40001001	A Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sãakpãmɩne nɩ nyã, wʋ yin a Nãa David nɩ Abraham bal pɔ,
40001002	Abraham lɛ ɩ Isaakɩ sãa, ka Isaakɩ mɩ ɩ Jekɔb sãa, ka Jekɔb mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ Juda sãa nɩ a wʋ yɛɛr,
40001003	ka Juda mɩ ɩ Perejɩ nɩ Jera sãa, ka ba ma di Tamar, nɩ Perejɩ na ɩ Hejoron sãa, ka Hejoron mɩ ɩ Aram sãa,
40001004	ka Aram mɩ ɩ Aminadab sãa, ka Aminadab mɩ ɩ Nason sãa, ka Nason mɩ ɩ Salmon sãa,
40001005	ka Salmon mɩ ɩ Boajɩ sãa, ka a wʋ ma di Worahab, ka Boajɩ mɩ ɩ Obed sãa, a wʋ ma lɛ Wʋruf, ka Obed mɩ ɩ Jesɩ sãa,
40001006	ka Jesɩ mɩ ɩ a Nãa David sãa. David lɛ ɩ a Solomon sãa, ka a wʋ ma dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a Yurɩya pɔɔ.
40001007	Ka a Solomon mɩ ɩ Wʋrehobom sãa, ka Wʋrehobom mɩ ɩ Abija sãa, ka Abija mɩ ɩ Asa sãa,
40001008	ka Asa mɩ ɩ Jehosafatɩ sãa, ka a Jehosafatɩ mɩ ɩ Jehoram sãa, ka Jehoram mɩ ɩ Yujiya sãa,
40001009	ka Yujiya mɩ ɩ Jotam sãa, ka Jotam mɩ ɩ Ahajɩ sãa, ka Ahajɩ mɩ ɩ Hɛjɩkiya sãa,
40001010	ka Hɛjɩkiya mɩ ɩ Manasɛ sãa, ka Manasɛ mɩ ɩ Amɔn sãa, ka Amɔn mɩ ɩ Josiya sãa,
40001011	ka Josiya mɩ ɩ Jekoniya sãa, nɩ a wʋ yɛɛr a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban bar a ba tẽe tɩ chen tɩ kpɩɛrɛ Babilon tẽe.
40001012	Ban wa tɩ be a Babilon tẽe pɔ, Jekoniya lɛ ɩ a Sealtɩɛl sãa, ka Sealtɩɛl ɩ Jerubabel sãa,
40001013	ka Jerubabel mɩ ɩ Abiud sãa, ka Abiud mɩ ɩ Eliyakim sãa, ka Eliyakim mɩ ɩ Ajor sãa,
40001014	ka Ajor mɩ ɩ Jadɔk sãa, ka Jadɔk mɩ ɩ Achɩm sãa, ka Achɩm mɩ ɩ Ɛliud sãa,
40001015	ka Ɛliud mɩ ɩ Elɩyajar sãa, ka Elɩyajar mɩ ɩ Matan sãa, ka Matan mɩ ɩ Jekɔb sãa,
40001016	Jekɔb mɩ lɛ ɩ a Josefʋ sãa na ɩ Mɛɛr sɩrɛ 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Yesu ma, a Yesu nyã lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
40001017	An yi Abraham tɩ ta a Nãa David, a Yesu sãakpãmɩne ɩ naa pie nɩ anaar, an yi Nãa David tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a ba dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃sɩ na nyɔɔr ba chiin a Babilon wɛr pɔ ba mɩ ɩ naa pie nɩ anaar, an lɛ yi a ba gbãgbaar ɩfʋ a Babilon wɛr pɔ tɩ tãn a Nɩ-iraa a ba mɩ ɩ pie nɩ anaar.
40001018	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto dɔɔfʋ yele tu. A wʋ ma Mɛɛr ŋmaan na Josefʋ baraa tɩchɛ baa kul taa sɛrɛ ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ vɛ̃ ka wʋ tara pʋɔ.
40001019	A wʋ baraa Josefʋ na ɩ nɩtor jũu, ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ su wʋ vĩ nɩyɔɔ pɔ ɛ, ka wʋ tɩɛr ɩka wʋ sɔɔl bar wʋ jaa jomm.
40001020	Wʋn wa tɩɛr a yele nyã maalfʋ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn malaka wa a wʋ sɛ̃ jãn pɔ wa 'yɛr, "Josefʋ, David bie, ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɩka fʋ de a Mɛɛr ka wʋ ɩ a fʋ pɔɔ ɛ, a bie na be a wʋ pʋɔm yin a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ.
40001021	Wʋn dɔɔn dabile ka fʋ na bʋɔlɔ a wʋ yuor Yesu, 'lɔ lɛ na faa a wʋ nɩbɛ yin a ba yeldɛbɛ pɔ."
40001022	Anyã a jaa ɩ naa ka a wiil a sɩ Soro 'yɛrbie wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr tu a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrɛ pɔ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ,
40001023	"Nyɛ a pɔɔsarbile na tara na pʋɔ dɔɔ dabile, ban 'yɔ̃ɔn a wʋ yuor Emanuwɛl," a par lɛ, Nãaŋmɩn ben a sɩ sɛ̃.
40001024	Josefʋ na wa jɛɔ a gʋ̃ɔ pɔ, wʋ ɩn a lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn malaka na 'yɛr ɩka wʋ ɩ. Ka wʋ de a Mɛɛr ka wʋ ɩ a wʋ pɔɔ,
40001025	tɩchɛ baa lɔɔ sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn dɔɔ a dabile, na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ yuor Yesu.
40002001	Yesu ban wa dɔɔ Bɛtɩlɛhɛm tẽe a Judiya paal pɔ a Nãa Hɛrɔd sɔ̃ɔ, yɛ̃ dẽme yin be a Jerusalɛm sapar wa,
40002002	na ba wa sʋrɔ, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ a bie be ban dɔɔ ka wʋ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa? Sɩ nyɛ naa a wʋ ŋmɛrbir a sapar ɩka sɩ wa puor wʋ."
40002003	A Nãa Hɛrɔd na wa wõ a lɛ wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa, ka Jerusalɛm nɩyɔɔ pʋʋr mɩ sɔ̃ɔ,
40002004	be lɛ wʋ bʋɔl a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe sʋʋr bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔ a jie 'lɔ ban na dɔɔ a Nɩ-iraa.
40002005	Ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Bɛtɩlɛhɛm na be Judiya, lɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ dɔ̃ɔ sɛb bin,
40002006	'Fʋ̃ʋ Bɛtɩlɛhɛm na be a Judiya paal pɔ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ jaa pʋʋrbile a Juda kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme pɔ, fʋ pɔ lɛ a kpɛ̃ɔ sʋɔ na yi kaara a n nɩbɛ Isɩral.' "
40002007	Be lɛ ka Hɛrɔd sɔɔl bʋɔl a yɛ̃ dẽme bala sʋʋr ba a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a ŋmɛrbir na pur wa.
40002008	Be lɛ wʋ tara ba chiin Bɛtɩlɛhɛm tɩ 'yɛr, "Yɩ chen tɩ yɔbɔ a bie kaa nɛ nɛ, yin wa nyɛ wʋ yɩ lɩɛb wa 'yɛr kʋ ma ka n mɩ chen tɩ puor wʋ."
40002009	Ban wa chɛl a nãa 'yɛr baar, ba yin lo a sɔr chiine, a ŋmɛrbir 'lɔ ban nyɛ a sapar de ban nie tɩ ara a jie 'lɔ a bie na be.
40002010	Ban wa nyɛ ka a ŋmɛrbir ara nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ban yɔɔ jaa.
40002011	Ban kpɛ a yir pɔ, ba nyɛn a bie nɩ a wʋ ma Mɛɛr, na ba gbur dumo puor wʋ. Be lɛ ba tũ a ba wʋʋr pɔ ir kʋfʋsɩ na ɩ sɛlma, nyɩnyɩbɩ kãa nyũu nʋ̃ɔ nɩ kãnyũu ala ban bʋɔlɔ sɩmura kʋ wʋ.
40002012	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ kpãa ba a jãn pɔ, ɩka ba ta lɛ lɩɛb chen a Nãa Hɛrɔd sɛ̃ ɛ, ka ba tu jiyuo kul a ba tẽe.
40002013	A yɛ̃ bɔ̃ɔnbɔ na wa chen baar, a Nãaŋmɩn malaka wan Josefʋ sɛ̃ jãn pɔ wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Vaa ir 'mɔɔ a bie nɩ a wʋ ma, na fʋ jo chiin be Ijipitɩ wɛr pɔ, na fʋ tɩ be a be wa tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn na 'yɛr kʋ fʋ, bojũu a Hɛrɔd nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ bʋɔrɔ na a bie kʋfʋ."
40002014	Ka a Josefʋ ir 'mɔɔ a bie nɩ a wʋ ma a tɩ̃sɔɔ bɩ̃ɩn jo chiin be a Ijipitɩ.
40002015	Be lɛ wʋ tɩ jɩ̃nɛ tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Nãa Hɛrɔd na wa kpi. A yelsɩ anyã ɩ naa lɛ ka a na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka a lɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛ'yɛrɛ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩka, "Ijipitɩ pɔ lɛ ɩn bʋɔl a n bie yin."
40002016	A Nãa Hɛrɔd na wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a yɛ̃ dẽme banyã na yɩ a sapar bɛl wʋ naa a suur kpɛ wʋ a wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ sojasɩ ɩka ba chen tɩ kʋ dabile jaa na be a Bɛtɩlɛhɛm na ta yuom ayi bɩɩ na ba ta sɛrɛ ɛ, yi a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa wʋn sʋʋr bɔ̃ɔn yi a yɛ̃ bɔ̃ɔnbɔ sɛ̃.
40002017	A lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Jeremiya na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ,
40002018	"Ba wõn kɔkɔr be a Wurama tẽe pɔ, kõyiel nɩ wuur kpɩ̃ɛn, Wurachɛl lɛ kõnõ a wʋ bibiir 'yɔ̃ɔ. Ba kpi na, waa lɛ bʋɔrɔ 'maalfʋ ɛ bojũu baa lɛ chɛnɛ go ɛ."
40002019	Hɛrɔd na wa kpi, Nãaŋmɩn malaka wan Josefʋ sɛ̃ be a Ijipitɩ jãn pɔ wa 'yɛr,
40002020	"Vaa ir 'mɔɔ a bie nɩ a wʋ ma na fʋ chiin a Isɩral wɛr pɔ, a bala na dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔrɔ a bie kʋfʋ kpi naa."
40002021	Josefʋ vaan ir 'mɔɔ a bie nɩ a wʋ ma chiin a Isɩral wɛr pɔ.
40002022	Tɩchɛ wʋn wa wõ ɩka Archelaus lɛ di a nãa a Judiya a wʋ sãa kũu puor, wʋ joro na dãbɩ̃ɛ ɩka wʋ lɛ chen a be. Ka a Nãaŋmɩn wa kpãa wʋ a jãn pɔ ɩka wʋ chen be Galilee paal pɔ.
40002023	Be lɛ wʋ chen Najaretɩ tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a be, ka a lɛ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, "Ban bʋɔl wʋ naa Najaretɩ nɩrɛ."
40003001	Sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Jɔɔn kɔ̃suor mʋɔlɔ a Judiya mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ
40003002	'yɛrɛ, "Yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ befʋ, a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ ta na."
40003003	Jɔɔn nyã 'yɛr lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Isaiya dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr, "Kɔkɔr kɔ̃ɔ lɛ gɔ̃nɔ̃ 'yɛrɛ be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ, chɔɔr a sɩ Soro sɔr, maal a wʋ sɔbie ka a tor."
40003004	Nyɔɔma kɔɔlʋ fuu lɛ Jɔɔn ma su tɩ de gãn a lũn a sɩɛ. Soor nɩ sɩkãa lɛ ɩ a wʋ bʋ̃diir.
40003005	Nɩyɔɔ yin a Jerusalɛm nɩ Judiya chiine a wʋ sɛ̃ nɩ a bala na yi a Jordan man koor.
40003006	Ba woro naa a ba yeldɛbɛ tɩ wʋ suoro ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ be a Jordan man pɔ.
40003007	Jɔɔn na wa nyɛ a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Saduseemɩne na waara a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ jie, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn waa bibiir, an n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka yɩ jo yi a Nãaŋmɩn suur na waara mɔ̃?
40003008	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ lɛ befʋ wiil ɩka yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr.
40003009	Yɩ ta chɛnɛ ŋmara jir 'yɔ̃ɔn yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɩka, 'Abraham lɛ ɩ a sɩ sãa ɛ.' N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ɔn maal a kʋsɩbɛ anyãna ka a lɩɛb ɩ a Abraham bibiir.
40003010	A 'lar dɔɔl a tɩɛ pĩlem gu a ŋmaafʋ, tɩɛ jaa ba wa wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃ sʋ̃n ɛ ban ŋmaa wʋn lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ bũu pɔ.
40003011	"Maa 'lɔ suoro yɩn nɩ kʋ̃ɔ ka yɩ na lɩɛb a yɩ befʋ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na tara kpɛ̃ɔ gar ma ben a n puor waara, a wʋ nafɔɔr gba ba sɛɛ ɩka n tuo ɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ na de a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nɩ bũu son yɩ.
40003012	A ŋmayɩɛlaa ben a wʋ nũu pɔ, ka wʋ na yɩɛl a mʋ̃ɩ a vafʋ jie na wʋ kpaar a bie 'yɔ̃ɔ a boor pɔ tɩ chʋm a sɔ̃sɔɔr nɩ bũu 'lɔ na ba tara kpĩinfʋ bar."
40003013	Yesu yin a be a Galilee chen a Jordan man pɔ, ka a Jɔɔn na tɩ so wʋ a kʋ̃ɔ.
40003014	Jɔɔn ba ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ so wʋ ɛ, na wʋ 'yɛr fʋ̃ʋ lɛ sɛɛ ɩka fʋ so ma tɩchɛ ka fʋ lɛ wa a n sɛ̃ go?
40003015	Tɩchɛ ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Vɛ̃ ka a ɩ a lɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã, a vɩɛl na ɩka sɩ ɩ a lɛ jaa Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ." Ka Jɔɔn sɔɔ lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr.
40003016	A lɛ wʋn wa so a Yesu a kʋ̃ɔ baar, a wʋ yi a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ wʋ nyɛ a saaju na yuo a wʋ nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na kaara ŋmam kaar suu wa mar a Yesu ju.
40003017	Tɩ a kɔkɔr yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ a saaju 'yɛrɛ, "A anyãna lɛ ɩ a n binʋ̃nãa ka a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ma 'maa nɩ wʋ."
40004001	A Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ tara na Yesu kpɛ̃n a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ, ka a tɩɩ tɩ bɛɛr wʋ kaa.
40004002	Waa di bon jaa ber lɩjaayi nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ gbulo lɩjaayi ɛ, ka kɔ̃ kpɛ wʋ.
40004003	A 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, 'yɛr kʋ a kʋsɩbɛ a nyãna ka a lɩɛb bʋ̃diir."
40004004	Tɩchɛ ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, bʋ̃diir tɛɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kʋ nɩrɛ nyɛvʋr ɛ, tɩchɛ 'yɛrbir jaa na yi Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ pɔ."
40004005	A bɛɛr kaa sʋɔ lɛ tara wʋn don a Jerusalɛm, tɩ wiil wʋ a puorfʋ jie na do gar a jaa,
40004006	tɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, ɔɔ lo a tẽe. A sɛb ɩka, wʋn vɛ̃n ka a wʋ malakasɩ gu fʋ na ba nyɔɔ fʋ nɩ a ba nuur ka fu gbɛr kʋ ŋme kʋsɩr ɛ."
40004007	Ka a Yesu mɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A mɩ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, ta bɛɛr a yɩ Nãaŋmɩn kaa ɛ."
40004008	A tɩɩ lɛ tara wʋn don tɔ̃ɔ ju tɩ wiil wʋ a nãa di jiir a jaa na be ka a wɛr pɔ, na a bʋ̃vɩɛlsɩ lɛ an be.
40004009	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ɩn kʋ fʋ naa anyãna a jaa, ala ɩ fʋ gbur dumo puor ma."
40004010	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ Satan nyã tɔɔ yi be. A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, a sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka yɩ puoro na yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a 'lɔ tɛɛ."
40004011	A tɩɩ bar wʋn tɩ chen, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn malakasɩ wa sʋ̃ʋ wʋ.
40004012	Yesu na wa wõ ɩka ba nyɔɔn Jɔɔn na ba pɔɔ, wʋ chen Galilee.
40004013	Wʋ yin Najaretɩ na wʋ tɩ kpɩɛrɛ be a Kapenahum a man nɛɛ be Jebulun nɩ Naftalɩ wɛr pɔ.
40004014	Ka a lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Isaiya na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ,
40004015	"Jebulun wɛr, Naftalɩ wɛr, a man sɔr a Jordan man gɔ̃ɔn. Galilee be a nɩyor na kpɩɛrɛ.
40004016	A nɩbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ be libe pɔ nyɛn chãa, nɩbɛ bala na ba dɔ̃ɔ tara nyɛvʋr Nãaŋmɩn pɔ ɛ, nyɛn Nãaŋmɩn chãa kpɛ̃ɛ."
40004017	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ Yesu piel na wʋ mʋɔlɔ 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ befʋ a saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ ta na."
40004018	Yesu na wa de a Galilee man gogoro lana, wʋ nyɛn yɛɛr ayi Simon ban bʋɔlɔ Pita nɩ a wʋ yɛbɛ Andiru na lɔɔrɔ lɔyaar 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ. Ba dɔ̃ɔ ɩ jɩ̃nyɔɔrbɔ.
40004019	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ turo ma, n vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ nyɔɔrɔ nɩbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
40004020	Ka ba tɔ̃ɔ tɩ̃ɛ a lɔyaarsɩ bar tɩ na ba turo wʋ.
40004021	Wʋn lɛ yɩ a be chiine, wʋ lɛ nyɛn yɛɛr ayi, Jemesɩ na ɩ Jebedee bidaba naa a wʋ yɛbɛ Jɔɔn ka ba be a gboro pɔ nɩ a ba sãa Jebedee, maala a ba lɔyaarsɩ ka wʋ bʋɔl ba.
40004022	A ba tɔ̃ɔ tɩɛ a gboro bar nɩ a ba sãa tɩ turo wʋ.
40004023	Yesu yɔn a Galilee wile ba a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir tɩ mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ tɩ sãana nɩrɛ jaa baal.
40004024	Ka a wʋ yele yaar a Siriya ka ba tara a baalsɩ ba jaa waan a wʋ sɛ̃, bala a baalsɩ nɩ ɩ̃gãn ɔbɔ na nyɔɔ, bala na tara a sɩdɛbɛ, banyã baal tãanaa na nyɔɔ nɩ gbɛrfʋ jaa bʋrɔ, ka wʋ sãa a ba baalsɩ.
40004025	Nɩyɔɔ yin Galilee, nɩ Dekapolisɩ, nɩ Jerusalɛm, nɩ Judiya nɩ a Jordan man gɔ̃ɔn wa turo wʋ.
40005001	Yesu na wa nyɛ a nɩyɔɔ, wʋ don tɔ̃ɔ ju, wʋn wa tɩ jɛ̃ baar ka a wʋ poturbo wa a wʋ sɛ̃.
40005002	A wʋ piel wile ba 'yɛrɛ,
40005003	"Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a yɩn banyãna na ba tara bon jaa ɛ, tɩ bʋɔrɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ. Yɩn lɛ so a saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ.
40005004	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a yɩn na kõnõ, Nãaŋmɩn na 'maan a yɩ nyãa.
40005005	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a yɩn na siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ. Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ ban bon jaa na be a wɛr pɔ.
40005006	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ banyã kɔ̃ nɩ kɔ̃nyũur na kpɛ yeltorsɩ jũu, ban tɩɩ naa.
40005007	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ yɩn banyã na kaara nɩrɛ nɩbaal, Nãaŋmɩn mɩ na kãan a yɩ nɩbaal.
40005008	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ banyã na nʋ̃ Nãaŋmɩn sɩrɛ, nɩ a ba nyãa wʋ jaa, bala lɛ na nyɛ Nãaŋmɩn.
40005009	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ banyã na bʋɔrɔ nyã'maar, ban bʋɔlɔ ban Nãaŋmɩn bibiir.
40005010	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ yɩn bala nɩbɛ na ge yeltorsɩ jũu, yɩn lɛ so a saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ.
40005011	"Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ yɩn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ nɩbɛ na tʋrɔ yɩ, na ba gere yɩ, tɩ ŋmara jirsɩ 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr dɛbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ yɩ, a maa jũu.
40005012	Yɩ tara pʋpɛl, a yɩ sãyar bɛrma naa a saaju, lɛ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ ge a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ be be.
40005013	"Yɩ kaara fɩka nyaar a wɛr pɔ, tɩchɛ a nyaar nʋ̃ɔ wa baar, ŋmɩnɛ ban lɛ ɩ wʋ ka wʋ lɛ nʋ̃mɔ̃ go? A maa lɛ tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ bon jaa ɛ, ba ma kpaar bar ka nɩbɛ nɛɛrɛ nɩ gbɛɛ.
40005014	"Yɩ kaara fɩka chãa a wɛr pɔ. Yir ban mɛ tɔ̃ɔ ju kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɔɔl ɛ.
40005015	Nɩrɛ maa chʋm fɩ̃tɩn de pɩɛ pɔɔ ɛ tɩchɛ wʋ ma bin a kuorgbe ju kʋ chaar yɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ jaa a yir pɔ.
40005016	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, yɩn lɛ ɩ chãa a yɩ taaba sɛ̃, ka ba na nyɛ a yɩ tʋ̃vɩɛlsɩ na ba pɛɛ a yɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na be a saaju.
40005017	"Yɩ ta tɩɛr ɩka n wan ɩka n wa sɔ̃ɔ a nɛbinãa bɩɩ, a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ wiilfʋ bar ɛ, n ba wa ɩka n wa sɔ̃ɔ yaa bar ɛ, n wan ɩka n vɛ̃ ka a ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
40005018	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ɩka a saaju nɩ a wɛr ba wa baar ɛ, a sɛbir bile bʋ̃'yen gba kʋ̃ ir a nɛbinãa pɔ ɛ, tɩ ta a lɛ yele jaa na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
40005019	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ jaa wa sɔ̃ɔ a nɛbinsɩ anyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tɩ wiil a wʋ taaba ka ba mɩ maala a lɛ, na ɩn a bile a saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ, tɩchɛ nyã jaa na maala tɩ wile bamɩne ka ba mɩ maala a lɛ, na ɩn kpɛ̃ɛ a saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
40005020	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, a yɩ yeltorsɩ ba wa tɩ gar a nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne ɛ, yɩn ba be na wa kpɛ a saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ.
40005021	"Yɩ wõn ban dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne, 'Ta kʋ nɩrɛ ɛ,' nɩrɛ nyã na kʋ nɩrɛ na nyɛn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ.
40005022	Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, ala ɩ fʋ nyɛn na yɛbɛ suur, wʋn nyɛn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ, ala ɩ fʋ tʋ̃n yɛbɛ na nyɛn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ a nɩbɛrɛ niem, fʋ̃ʋ wa 'yɛr nɩrɛ ɩka, jɔl nyã, na kpɛ̃n a bũu dagel 'lɔ pɔ.
40005023	"Ala wa ɩ fʋ waara nɩ naa a fʋ kʋfʋ, a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie na fʋ wa tɩɛr tɔ ɩka fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a yɛbɛ tara na 'yɛr,
40005024	bar a fʋ bon a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie tɩ lɩɛb chen tɩ 'maal a fʋ yɛbɛ tɩ pãa wa de a fʋ bon kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn.
40005025	"An ɩ yɩn nɩ a yɩ sãn sʋɔ lɛ chiine a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie, yɩ mʋlɔ wʋ a sɔr pɔ, ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, wʋn de yɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ a 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ nũu pɔ, ka wʋ de yɩ kʋ a nɩpɔɔraa ka wʋ mɩ pɔɔ yɩ bar.
40005026	Ala be a lɛ, faa be na wa yi ka fʋ̃ʋ ba wa yab a sãn baar ɛ.
40005027	"Yɩ dɔ̃ɔ wõ ban 'yɛr ɩka ta gãn nɩrɛ pɔɔ bɩɩ sɩrɛ ɛ.
40005028	Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ nyã jaa na wa kaa pɔɔ jaa tɩ̃ɩɩ tɩ bʋɔrɔ na gãn wʋ, a nɩrɛ 'lɔ gãn wʋ naa a wʋ tɩɛr pɔ.
40005029	Ala ɩ a fʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ nɩbir vɛ̃ naa ka fʋ ɩ yelbier, 'loo wʋ bar, a fʋ ɩ̃gãn lõboor ɩ̃sʋɔ na ba be be ɛ, sa naa a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa na kpɛ bũu pɔ.
40005030	Ala ɩ a fʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ nũu mɩ lɛ vɛ̃ ka fʋ ɩ yelbier ɛ, ŋmaa wʋ 'lɔ bar, a fʋ ɩ̃gãn lõboor ɩ̃sʋɔ na ba be be ɛ, sa naa a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa na kpɛ bũu pɔ.
40005031	"A mɩ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩka, nɩrɛ nyã jaa na tɔr a wʋ pɔɔ bar, wʋ kʋ wʋ a pɔɔ bar gãn.
40005032	Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, nɩrɛ nyã jaa na tɔr a wʋ pɔɔ bar, ala baa ɩ wʋ sɛ̃nɛ naa ɛ, vɛ̃n kʋ ɩ sɛ̃sɛ̃nɛ, nɩrɛ nyã jaa na kul a pɔɔ 'lɔ mɩ ɩn sɛ̃sɛ̃nɛ.
40005033	"Yɩ mɩ lɛ wõn ban dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne, 'Yɩ taa sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nɛɛ 'lɔ yɩn põl 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ tara a lɛ yɩn põl 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro.'
40005034	Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ ta pɔ jaa ɛ, yɩ ta pɔn a saaju gba ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn jaa jie lɛ,
40005035	bɩɩ a wɛr ju, a wʋ gbɛr dɔɔlfʋ jie lɛ bɩɩ Jerusalɛm ɛ, bojũu be lɛ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ kpɩɛrɛ.
40005036	Ta pɔn a fʋ ju ɛ, fʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka a fʋ jukɔɔl ɩ̃sʋɔ pɛl bɩɩ sɔb ɛ.
40005037	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ ɔ̃ɔ ɩ ɔ̃ɔ ka a yɩ kai ɩ kai, bon 'lɔ na gar a nɩtɔ̃ yin a dɛɛr sʋɔ sɛ̃.
40005038	"Yɩ dɔ̃ɔ wõ ban 'yɛr ɩka nɩbir na yãan nɩbir sãn, ka nyɩm mɩ yaa nyɩm sãn.
40005039	Tɩchɛ maa 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, ta pii a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔ̃ɔ fʋ sɔr ɛ. Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ wa 'ma fʋ a tʋkpal nyã pɔ, lɩɛb a nyã lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ.
40005040	Ka nɩrɛ wa bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ sɛb fʋ nãa yir tɩ de a fʋ fuu, kʋ wʋ a 'lɔ fʋn su, na fʋ yaa a pʋɔm bon pʋɔ wʋ.
40005041	Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ wa fɩr fʋ ɩka fʋ de a wʋ tuor tuo chiin niem bɩ̃lãa, tuo chiin tɛɛr jaa.
40005042	Kʋ nɩrɛ jaa na sʋɔr fʋ, ta mɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ nyã mɩ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ pɛ̃ɛ a fʋ bon ɛ.
40005043	"Yɩ wõn ban dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩka, yɩ nʋ̃ a yɩ tɔ sʋɔ tɩ 'laar a yɩ dɔ̃sʋɔ.
40005044	Tɩchɛ maa 'lɔ 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, nʋ̃ a yɩ dɔ̃dẽme tɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ a bala na gere yɩ,
40005045	ka yɩ na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bibiir bojũu 'lɔ lɛ ma vɛ̃ ka a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ pur 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɩdɛbɛ nɩ a nɩsʋ̃n tɩ na wʋ ma vɛ̃ ka saa wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na tor nɩ a bala na ba tor ɛ.
40005046	Yɩn nʋ̃ a bala na nʋ̃ yɩ tɛɛ, bo sãyar lɛ yɩn nyɛ? A lõpodierbe maa mɩ ɩ a lɛ bɩɩ?
40005047	Yɩn ma puoro a bala tɛɛ na ɩ a yɩ nɩbɛ, bo tɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ be be? A bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, maa mɩ ɩ a lɛ bɩɩ?
40005048	Yɩ ɩ nɩmɩn a lɛ a yɩ sãa Nãaŋmɩn na be a saaju kaar.
40006001	"Yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, na yɩ taa mʋɔlɔ a yɩ yeltorsɩ a nɩbɛ niem ɛ, ka ba na bɔ̃ɔn ɛ, yɩn wa ɩrɛ a lɛ, yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ sãyar a yɩ sãa Nãaŋmɩn na be a saaju sɛ̃ ɛ.
40006002	"A lɛ jũu, fʋ̃ʋ wa de bon kʋ nɩrɛ na ba tara ɛ, ta vɛ̃ ka nɩbɛ bɔ̃ɔn ɛ, fɩka lɛ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme na ma maala a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie nɩ a tẽn pɔ ɛ, ka nɩbɛ na pɛɛ ba ɛ. Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, bala nyɛn a ba sãyar baar.
40006003	A lɛ jũu, fʋ̃ʋ wa de bon kʋ nɩrɛ na ba tara ɛ, ta vɛ̃ ka a gubaa nũu bɔ̃ɔn a bon 'lɔ a nũsʋ̃ɔ na maala ɛ,
40006004	ka nɩrɛ ta bɔ̃ɔn a bon fʋn maala ɛ, tɩchɛ a fʋ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na nyɛrɛ yelsɔɔlsɩ na kʋ fʋn a sãyar.
40006005	"Yɩn maa wa sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn, yɩ ta ma kaara a nɛɛr ayi dẽme kaar ɛ, ba ma nʋ̃n ɩka ba puoro a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie pɔ, nɩ a tẽbɛrɛ pɔ, nɩ a sɔchara pɔ, ka nɩbɛ na nyɛ ba. Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ɩka ba nyɛn a ba sãyar baar.
40006006	Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ maa wa sʋɔrɔ a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nyã sɩn ba nyɛrɛ ɛ, kpɛ a fʋ die pɔ, tɩ pɔɔ a pãn, tɩ sʋɔr a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na nyɛrɛ bon jaa, na yab fʋn a sãyar.
40006007	Yɩn maa wa sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn, yɩ ta ma 'yɛrɛ 'yɛrbie ala na ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, lɛ lɛ a bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ma maala, ba tɩɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na wõn a ba sʋɔrfʋ a ba 'yɛrbiyɔɔ jũu.
40006008	Yɩ ta kaara a ba kaar ɛ, a yɩ Sãa den nie bɔ̃ɔn bon 'lɔ yɩn bʋɔrɔ.
40006009	"Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ yɩn ma sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn. Sɩ Sãa na be a saaju. Sɩ kʋ naa a fʋ yuor tɩɩr.
40006010	A fʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ wʋ wa. A fʋ bɔfʋ wʋ ɩ a wɛr pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a fʋ bɔfʋ na ɩrɛ be a saaju.
40006011	Kʋ sɩ a dɩna bʋ̃diir ka a sɛɛn sɩ.
40006012	Vɛ̃ a sɩ yeldɛbɛ bar, nɩtãa lɛ sɩn ma vɛ̃ kʋ a sɩ taaba yeldɛbɛ bar ba.
40006013	Ta sɔɔ ka bɛɛr kaa nyɔɔ sɩ ɛ, faa sɩ yin a dɛɛr sʋɔ nũu pɔ.
40006014	"Yɩn wa vɛ̃ a yɩ taaba yeldɛbɛ bar ba, a yɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na be a saaju mɩ na vɛ̃n bar yɩ.
40006015	Yɩn ba wa vɛ̃ a yɩ taaba yeldɛbɛ kʋ ba ɛ, a yɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn mɩ kʋ̃ vɛ̃ a yɩ yeldɛbɛ kʋ yɩ ɛ.
40006016	"Yɩn wa gal kɔ̃, yɩ ta sɔ̃ a yɩ nin a nɛɛr ayi dẽme kaar ɛ, ba ma sɔ̃n a ba nin ka a ba taaba nyɛ bɔ̃ɔ ka ba gal kɔ̃. Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka ba nyɛn a ba sãyar baar.
40006017	Yɩn wa gal kɔ̃, yɩ lor a yɩ nie maal a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ,
40006018	ka nɩbɛ ta bɔ̃ɔn yɩn gal kɔ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nyã sɩn ba nyɛrɛ ɛ, a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nyã na nyɛrɛ yelsɔɔlsɩ na yab yɩn a sãyar.
40006019	"Yɩ ta bine a yɩ nãbonsɩ ka a wɛr ju be kpolo, nɩ sɔrɔ, nɩ na sɔ̃ɔ bar ɛ, nɩ be nãnyisɩ nɩ naa kpɛ ju ɛ.
40006020	Tɩchɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ nãbonsɩ bine a saaju, be lɛ a kpolo nɩ sɔrɔ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɔ̃ɔ bar ɛ, nɩ be a nãnyisɩ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ju ɛ.
40006021	A jie 'lɔ a fʋ nãbonsɩ na be, be lɛ a fʋ tɩɛr mɩ ma be.
40006022	"A fʋ nɩbir lɛ ɩ a fʋ ɩ̃gãn chãa. A fʋ nɩbir wa ɩ a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa ma sɛɛn na chãa.
40006023	Tɩchɛ a fʋ nɩbir ba wa ɩ ɛ, a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa ma ɩn libe. Ala ɩ a chãa 'lɔ na be a fʋ pɔ ɩn libe, nyɛ lɛ a libe na jɩ̃.
40006024	"Nɩrɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ nɩbɛrɛ ayi tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ. Wʋn nʋ̃n ɩ̃sʋɔ, tɩ 'laar ɩ̃sʋɔ, bɩɩ wõnõ a ɩ̃sʋɔ toor, tɩ ba wõnõ ɩ̃sʋɔ toor ɛ. Yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ libie ɛ.
40006025	"A lɛ jũu, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a yɩ nyɛvʋr yele wõnõ yɩ ka yɩ 'yɛrɛ ɩka, bo lɛ yɩn di, bɩɩ bo lɛ yɩn nyũ ɛ. Bɩɩ waala ɩka, bo lɛ yɩn su pɔɔ a ɩ̃gãn ɛ. A nyɛvʋr ba fɛr gar a bʋ̃diir ɛ, ka a ɩ̃gãn mɩ fɛr gar a bʋ̃sursɩ ɛ?
40006026	Yɩ kaa a lubil na be a saaju. Ba maa bʋr ɛ, bɩɩ ŋma ɛ, bɩɩ tara boor ma bin ɛ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ guolo ba. Yaa fɛr gar a lubil bɩɩ?
40006027	A yɩ buor sʋɔ lɛ na waal na wʋ tʋ̃ɔ de bɩbir bʋ̃'yen pʋɔ a wʋ nyɛvʋr pɔ?
40006028	"Ka bo lɛ vɛ̃ ka yɩ tɩɛrɛ a bʋ̃sursɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ? Yɩ kaa nyɛ a mɔpuul lɛ an ma nʋ̃ɔ, ba maa tʋ̃ ɛ, bɩɩ wob fuu su ɛ,
40006029	a Nãa Solomon gba nɩ a wʋ tɩɩr wʋ jaa ba dɔ̃ɔ su fuu ka wʋ vɩɛlɛ gar a mɔpuul a nyãna ɛ.
40006030	Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn maal a mɔpuul ka a vɩɛlɛ, tɩchɛ a maa kor ɛ. Nɩbɛ ma chʋm ka a di. A Nãaŋmɩn na ma maal a mɔpuul a nɩtɔ̃, wʋ kaara a yɩn na ɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ gar a mɔpuul anyãna. A yɩ sɔɔfʋ lɛ ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ.
40006031	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta waala 'yɛrɛ ɩka, bo lɛ yɩn di bɩɩ nyũ ɛ, bɩɩ bo lɛ yɩn su ɛ?
40006032	A bala na ba puor ɛ, lɛ de a ba tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a anyãna pɔ, a yɩ Sãa bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka yɩ bʋɔrɔ naa a bonsɩ anyãna a jaa.
40006033	Yɩ de nie bɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nɩ a wʋ yeltorsɩ, tɩchɛ a anyãna a jaa, wʋn den pʋɔ yɩ.
40006034	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta waala a bio 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, bio lɛ na waala a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ. Bɩbir jaa tara na a wʋ yelwõnsɩ.
40007001	"Yɩ ta tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn mɩ wa tɔɔr a yɩ 'yɛr ɛ.
40007002	Nãaŋmɩn na tɔɔr a yɩ 'yɛr nɩtãa lɛ yɩn tɔɔr a yɩ tɔ sʋɔ 'yɛr. Lɛ fʋn man tɩr, lɛ mɩ lɛ ban man kʋ fʋ.
40007003	"Ŋmɩnɛ a fʋ nyɛ dabile na be a fʋ yɛbɛ nɩbir pɔ tɩ ba chɛlɛ a dakpɛ̃ɛ na be a fʋ̃ʋ nɩbir pɔ ɛ?
40007004	Bɩɩ ŋmɩnɛ fʋn ɩ 'yɛr kʋ a fʋ yɛbɛ vɛ̃ ka ir a dabile na be a fʋ nɩbir pɔ bar tɩ ba chɛlɛ a dakpɛ̃ɛ na be a fʋ nɩbir pɔ ɛ?
40007005	Yɩn nɛɛr ayi dẽme, de nie ir a dakpɛ̃ɛ a fʋ nɩbir pɔ bar na fʋ pãa nyɛrɛ tʋ̃ɔ ir a dabile a fʋ yɛbɛ nɩbir pɔ mɩ bar.
40007006	"Ta de bon na ɩ chɛchɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ baar ɛ, bɩɩ lɔb a fʋ bʋ̃vɩɛlsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ dor ɛ, ban nɛb na nɩ gbɛɛ tɩ lɩɛb nyɔɔ fʋ.
40007007	"Yɩ sʋɔr, Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ yɩ naa. Yɩ yɔbɔ, yɩn nyɛ naa, yɩ kpoor a pãn, wʋn yuo naa.
40007008	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sʋɔr na nyɛ naa, ka a 'lɔ mɩ na yɔbɔ nyɛ, ka a pãn mɩ yuo kʋ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kpoor.
40007009	"A yɩn na ɩ a sãamɩne, buor sʋɔ bie lɛ na sʋɔr a wʋ sãa bʋ̃diir, ka wʋ de kʋsɩr kʋ wʋ?
40007010	Bɩɩ ka a bie sʋɔr jɩ̃m, ka wʋ de waa kʋ wʋ?
40007011	Ala ɩ a yɩn na ɩ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ bɔ̃ɔn bʋ̃vɩla ma maal kʋ a yɩ bibiir, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an ɩ ka a yɩ Sãa na be a saaju, kʋ̃ de bʋ̃vɩɛl kʋ a bala na sʋɔr wʋ ɛ?
40007012	A lɛ yɩn ma bʋɔrɔ ɩka a nɩbɛ ba ma maala kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ mɩ ma maala a lɛ ban bʋɔrɔ kʋrɔ ba, a nyã lɛ ɩ a Nɛbinãa nɩ a 'Yɛ'yɛrbɛ Wiilfʋ.
40007013	"Yɩ tu a dɔ̃dɔr fɩɩl pɔ kpɛ, bojũu a dɔ̃dɔr yal sɔr ɩn jaa kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ tɩ ɩ sɔ̃ɔfʋ sɔr tɩchɛ ka nɩyɔɔ turo.
40007014	A dɔ̃dɔr ɩn jaa fɩɩl ka nyɛvʋr sɔr mɩ ɩ jaa kãrakãra ka nɩbɛ bɩ̃lãa na tʋ̃ɔ tu.
40007015	"Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a jire 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ, ba ma bal ba mɩ̃ɛ piir kaar tɩchɛ ba ɩn mɔdʋ̃ be be na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
40007016	A ba wɔ̃mɔ̃ lɛ yɩn bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban be. Ba ma pɔr 'wɔ̃rɔ gʋtɩɛ ju bɩɩ pɔr kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ nyaartɩɛ ju ɔ?
40007017	Lɛ mɩ lɛ tɩsʋ̃ jaa ma wɔ̃n wɔ̃sʋ̃n ka tɩdɛɛr mɩ ma wɔ̃ wɔ̃dɛbɛ.
40007018	Tɩsʋ̃ ba wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃dɛbɛ ɛ bɩɩ tɩdɛɛr mɩ ba wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃sʋ̃n ɛ.
40007019	Tɩɛ jaa baa wa wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃sʋ̃n ɛ, ban ŋmaa wʋn lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ bũu pɔ.
40007020	A ba wɔ̃mɔ̃ lɛ yɩn de bɔ̃ɔn ba.
40007021	"A ba ɩ nɩrɛ jaa na bʋɔlɔ ɩka n Soro, n Soro, lɛ na kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ nyã na maala a lɛ a n Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na be a saaju na bʋɔrɔ.
40007022	A bɩbir 'lɔ daar, nɩyɔɔ na 'yɛr kʋ ma n Soro, n Soro, saa 'yɛr Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr a fʋ yuor pɔ ɛ, na sɩ diin a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yɩ a fʋ yuor pɔ ɛ, na sɩ tʋ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ a fʋ yuor pɔ ɛ?
40007023	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩn 'yɛr kʋ ba, n ba bɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɛ, yɩ tɔɔ chen be, yɩn yelbe-ɩrbɛ.
40007024	"A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ jaa na wõ a n 'yɛrbie anyãna tɩ maala a lɛ na kaara fɩka yɛ̃ sʋɔ na mɛ a wʋ yir dɔɔl pie ju.
40007025	Saa wa naa, ka a kʋ̃ɔ yɩ yaar jilʋ̃ a yir ka a sɛsɛbɛ fu ŋme a yir tɩchɛ waa lo ɛ, bojũu wʋ ara na kʋsɩr ju.
40007026	Tɩchɛ, nɩrɛ jaa na wõ a n 'yɛrbie anyãna tɩ na waa maal ɛ, kaara fɩka jɔl na mɛ a wʋ yir dɔɔl bire ju.
40007027	Saa wa naa, ka a kʋ̃ɔ yɩ yaar jilʋ̃ a yir, ka a sɛsɛbɛ fu ŋme a yir kʋ lo ka a wʋ lofʋ ɩ dɛɛr."
40007028	Yesu na wa 'yɛr a 'yɛrbie anyãna baar nɛɛ 'maan a nɩyɔɔ nɩ a wʋ wiilfʋ,
40007029	bojũu wʋ wile ban nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ gar a ba nɛbinãa wiwiilbe.
40008001	Yesu na wa yɩ a tɔ̃ɔ ju suu nɩyɔɔ turo wʋ naa,
40008002	a nɩyɔɔ na turo wʋ, ka daba ɩ̃sʋɔ na tara kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ baal wa gbur dumo a wʋ niem tɩ 'yɛr, "N Soro fʋ̃ʋ sɔɔ sãa ma."
40008003	Ka Yesu tur a wʋ nũu sɩɩr a daba tɩ 'yɛr, "N sɔɔ naa, sa." Ajienaa ka a daba kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ baal bar wʋ.
40008004	Be lɛ ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, taa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ chen tɩ wiil a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrloro na fʋ chiin a fʋ kʋfʋ tɩ ir a nɛɛ 'lɔ a Mosesɩ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ka a di dãasɩɛ.
40008005	Yesu na wa kpɛ a Kapenahum a sojasɩ nɩdiere chen a wʋ sɛ̃ tɩ sʋɔr wʋ 'yɛr,
40008006	"N Soro, a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ lɛ gã a yir ba tʋɔrɔ ire ɛ, na wʋ wõnõ a ɩ̃gãn tuo."
40008007	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ɩ̃n wa sa naa a wʋ baal kʋ wʋ."
40008008	Ka a sojasɩ nɩdiere 'yɛr, "N Soro n ba sɛɛ ɩka fʋ wa a n yir ɛ, 'yɛr a 'yɛrbir tɛɛ, a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ na sa naa.
40008009	A maa mɩ̃ɛ tara na nɩbɛrɛ ɩn joro dãbɩ̃ɛ, naa mɩ tara a sojasɩ ka ba mɩ be a n pĩlem, maa 'yɛr kʋ nyã ɩka wʋ, chen, wʋ ma chen naa, bɩɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩka, wa, wʋ ma wa naa, bɩɩ ka n 'yɛr kʋ a n gbãgbaa, maal nyã, wʋ ma maal naa."
40008010	Yesu na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃, nɛɛ 'maa wʋ naa ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a bala na turo wʋ, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ. A Isɩral nɩbɛ pɔ gba, n ba nyɛ a sɔɔfʋ nyã tɔ ɛ.
40008011	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka nɩyɔɔ na yin jie jaa wa na ba wa lɔ̃ɔ din a Abraham nɩ a Isaakɩ nɩ a Jekɔb a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ,
40008012	tɩchɛ a bala na so a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ, wʋn lɔb ban bar yõo a jilibe pɔ, be lɛ ban kõnõ ɔɔrɔ nɩ nyɩmɛ."
40008013	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a sojasɩ nɩdiere, "Kulo, a ɩ a lɛ kʋ fʋ, fʋn tara a sɔɔfʋ jũu." A tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ sa naa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ.
40008014	Yesu na kpɛ a Pita yir, wʋ nyɛn a Pita dɩ̃ɛ ma ɩ̃gãn na tɔ kʋ gã.
40008015	Wʋ sɩɩr a pɔɔ nũu, ka a ɩ̃gãn tʋl baar a wʋ ir maal bʋ̃diir kʋ wʋ.
40008016	A jãanʋɔr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ba waan na nɩyɔɔ a sɩdɛbɛ na tara a Yesu sɛ̃, ka wʋ de a 'yɛrbir diin a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi tɩ sãa a bala jaa an ɔɔrɔ.
40008017	Ka a lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Isaiya na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, "Ɩka wʋ den a sɩn baalsɩ a jaa bar."
40008018	Yesu na wa nyɛ a nɩyɔɔ na ŋmaa jilʋ̃ wʋ, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo yɩ gɔ̃ɔ a man gɔ̃ɔn.
40008019	A nɛɛ wiwiilbe ɩ̃sʋɔ tɔɔn ta wʋ tɩ 'yɛr, "Wiwile, jie jaa fʋn chiine ɩn turo fʋ naa."
40008020	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Mɔbaar tara naa bɔɔr ka lubil mɩ tara choor tɩchɛ maa Nɩsaal Bie ba tara jie na bin a n ju ɛ."
40008021	Ka a wʋ poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N Soro kʋ ma sɔr ka n kul tɩ ũu a n sãa baar."
40008022	Tɩchɛ ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a daba, "Turo ma tɩ bar ka a kũn ũno a ba mɩ̃ɛ kũn."
40008023	Yesu na wa kpɛ a gboro pɔ a wʋ poturbo mɩ tu wʋn kpɛ.
40008024	Kɔ̃sɛbɛ ir a man pɔ, ka a gboro sɛɛ kʋ̃ɔ ɩrɛ na mʋr tɩchɛ ka a Yesu gã gur.
40008025	Be lɛ ba chen tɩ sɩ̃ɩ wʋ na ba 'yɛr, "Sɩ Soro faa sɩ, a kʋ̃ɔ dire sɩ naa!"
40008026	Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Bo lɛ so ka yɩ joro a dãbɩ̃ɛ? A yɩ sɔɔfʋ lɛ ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ." Ka a Yesu ir tãn ka a sɛsɛbɛ na ta furo ŋmaa vʋʋr ka a kʋ̃ɔ mɩ na ta ɔɔrɔ lo jaa jomm.
40008027	Nɛɛ 'maan a nɩbɛ ka ba sʋrɔ taa, nɩ an lɛ a nyã ka a sɛsɛbɛ nɩ a kʋ̃ɔ tu a wʋ nɛɛ?
40008028	Yesu na wa ta a Gadara paal pɔ, dɔɔr ayi na tara sɩdɛbɛ yɩn a yar par tuor wʋ. Ban ɩ a nɩbebe jũu, nɩrɛ jaa maa 'la tu a sɔr 'lɔ ɛ.
40008029	Ban wa nyɛ a Yesu ba ŋmen chɛlma tɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Bo lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ ka a sɩ sɛ̃, fʋ̃ʋ Nãaŋmɩn Bie? Fʋ wan ɩka fʋ wa ge sɩ tɩchɛ ka a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ bɩbir wa ta bɩɩ?"
40008030	Do yɔɔ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ara gbʋr ba dire.
40008031	Ka a sɩdɛbɛ sʋɔr wʋ, "Ala ɩ fʋn dii sɩn bar, sɔɔ ka sɩ chen tɩ kpɛ a dor anyã pɔ."
40008032	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen!" Be lɛ a sɩdɛbɛ yi naa kpɛ a dor pɔ, ka a dor a jaa jo tĩgbil suu tɩ kpɛ a man kʋ̃ɔ pɔ gbʋ̃m kpi kpi.
40008033	A bala na kaara a dor jon kul, ban wa tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a tẽe pɔ, ba man bon 'lɔ jaa na ɩ a bala na tara a sɩdɛbɛ nɩ a lɛ jaa na ɩ a dor.
40008034	A tẽe wʋ jaa nɩbɛ yɩn wa a Yesu sɛ̃; ban wa nyɛ wʋ ba sʋɔr wʋn ɩka wʋ yɩ a ba wɛr pɔ.
40009001	Yesu na wa kpɛ a gboro pɔ, wʋ gɔ̃ɔn a man chen a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tẽe be a Kapenahum.
40009002	Dɔɔr bamɩne tuon daba nɩ fɔbaa nuur nɩ a gbɛɛ na kpi waan wa kpɛ̃n wʋ gaal a Yesu niem. Yesu na wa nyɛ lɛ ban sɔɔ de wʋ, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a baalaa, "N bie ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, a fʋ yeldɛbɛ vɛ̃n bar."
40009003	Ka a nɛɛ wiwiilbe bamɩne pãa jɛ̃ bʋlɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ pʋʋr pɔ, "A daba nyã fere na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn yuor."
40009004	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban tɩɛr, ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tɩɛrɛ dɛɛr a yɩ pʋʋr pɔ?
40009005	'Yɛr buor sʋɔ lɛ ɩ kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃? N 'yɛr ɩka a wʋ yeldɛbɛ vɛ̃n bar bɩɩ n 'yɛr ɩka wʋ ir chiine?
40009006	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã ɩn wiil yɩ naa ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka maa Nɩsaal Bie tara na kpɛ̃ɔ a wɛr pɔ, na vɛ̃ nɩrɛ yeldɛbɛ bar." Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a gbɛrɛ, "Ir 'mɔɔ a fʋ bʋ̃gãnaa kulo nɩ."
40009007	Ka a daba vaa ir kulo.
40009008	A nɩbɛ na nyɛ a lɛ nɛɛ 'maa ban ka ba pɛɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ nɩsaal a kpɛ̃ɔ nyã.
40009009	Yesu na wa yi a be chiine, wʋ nyɛn daba na di Matiu na jɩ̃nɛ a lõpoo defʋ jie, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ir turo ma," ka a Matiu ir turo wʋ.
40009010	Ka ba 'mataa kul a wʋ yir tɩ jɛ̃ dire ka a lõpodiere nɩ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ yɔɔ wa pʋɔ ba nɩ a Yesu poturbo ka ba 'mataa dire.
40009011	A Faraseemɩne na wa nyɛ a nɩtɔ̃ ba sʋʋr a Yesu poturbo, "Bo lɛ so ka a yɩ wiwile 'mataa dire nɩ a lõpodierbe nɩ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ?"
40009012	Yesu wõn a lɛ ban 'yɛr, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩrɛ na kpɛ̃mɛ ba chiine tɩtɩlɛ jie ɛ, tɩchɛ baalaa lɛ ma chen.
40009013	Tɩchɛ yɩ kul tɩ tɩɛr a yele nyã kaa, 'N bʋɔrɔ na nɩbaal a ba ɩ dʋ̃n bɔɔr lofʋ ɛ.' N ba wa ɩka n wa bʋɔl a bala na tor ɛ, tɩchɛ n wan ɩka n wa bʋɔl a yelbe-ɩrbɛ."
40009014	Ka a Jɔɔn poturbo wa a wʋ sɛ̃ wa sʋrɔ, "Ŋmɩnɛ a sɩn nɩ a Faraseemɩne ma gal kɔ̃ tɩchɛ ka a fʋ poturbo 'lɔ maa gal kɔ̃ ɛ?"
40009015	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Fʋn tʋ̃ɔ maal a bala ban bʋɔl a pɔɔ paalaa jie ka ba tara pʋsɔ̃ɔ a pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ na chɛnɛ be a ba sɛ̃ ɔ, ban tʋ̃ɔ naa? Sɔ̃ɔ waara naa ka a nɩbɛ na wa nyɔɔ ma chiin, a ber ala pɔ lɛ a n poturbo pʋɔ na sɔ̃ɔ ka ba gal kɔ̃.
40009016	"Nɩrɛ maa ŋmaa fɔpaalaa sɛ choo fɔkoraa pɔ ɛ, 'lɔ be ɩ a lɛ a fɔpaalaa na tɔɔn a fɔkoraa chɩɛr. Ka a chɩɛrfʋ na ɩ dɛɛr.
40009017	Bɩɩ nɩrɛ ma den dãbɩ̃ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ dãa wɔkoraa pɔ ɛ, 'lɔ be ɩ a lɛ a dãbɩ̃ɩn na pur naa a wʋɔ ka a dãa kpaar ka a wʋɔ mɩ sɔ̃ɔ. Ba ma den dãbɩ̃ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ a dãa wɔpaalaa pɔ, ka a ta sɔ̃ɔ ɛ."
40009018	A Yesu na chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ a anyãna kʋrɔ ba, a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir nɩdiere wa gbur dumo a wʋ niem tɩ 'yɛr, "A n bipɔɔ lɛ kpi ajienaa, wa lɩɛb a fʋ nuur sɩɩr wʋ tɩ wʋn sa naa."
40009019	Ka a Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo ir turo wʋ.
40009020	Ban wa de a sɔr chiine ka pɔɔ na lo sɩɛ suoro faara yuom pie nɩ ayi, wʋ gʋɔr a Yesu puor tɩ sɩɩr a fuu nɛɛ,
40009021	bojũu wʋ tɩɛr a wʋ pʋɔm ɩka 'lɔ sɩɩr a Yesu fuu wʋn sa naa.
40009022	Yesu na lɩɛb nyɛ a pɔɔ wʋ 'yɛr naa, "Ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ n yɛpɔɔ, a fʋ sɔɔfʋ sãa fʋ naa." A dẽdẽe daa a pɔɔ jɩ̃ɩ ŋmaa naa.
40009023	A Yesu na wa kpɛ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩdiere yir na wʋ nyɛ a ɩɩlpɛɛlbɛ nɩ a nɩyɔɔ na pɔɔrɔ gɔ̃mɔ̃,
40009024	ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ tɔɔ chen be a pɔɔbile ba kpi ɛ, wʋ gur naa." Ka ba laara wʋ.
40009025	A nɩyɔɔ na wa yɩ a yõo baar, wʋ kpɛ̃n tɩ nyɔɔ a wʋ nũu, ka a pɔɔbile vaa ir.
40009026	Ka a yele ŋme yaar a paal 'lɔ wʋ jaa.
40009027	Yesu na wa yi a be chiine, jɔ̃n ayi turo wʋ naa, na ba gboolo bʋɔlɔ, "Kaa sɩ nɩbaal, David Bie."
40009028	Wʋn wa kpɛ a yir, a jɔ̃n wan a wʋ sɛ̃, ka Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Yɩ sɔɔn de ɩka ɩn tʋ̃ɔ sa a yɩ baal ɔ?" Ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ɔ̃ɔ, sɩ Soro."
40009029	Ka wʋ sɩɩr a ba nɩbie tɩ 'yɛr, "A yɩ sɔɔfʋ jũu yɩn nyɛrɛ naa."
40009030	Ka a ba nɩbie tɔ̃ɔ yuo yuor. Tɩchɛ ka Yesu kpãkpãan ba ɩka ba taa vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa bɔ̃ɔn ɛ.
40009031	Tɩchɛ ba yin tɩ ŋme a wʋ yele yaar a tẽe 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ wʋ jaa.
40009032	A jɔ̃n ayi bala na wa lɩɛb chen baar, ba tara na daba na tara sɩdɛbɛ na wʋ ɩ wõo waan a Yesu sɛ̃.
40009033	A sɩdɛbɛ na wa yɩ a daba pɔ baar, wʋ piel 'yɛrɛ, ka nɛɛr 'maa a nɩyɔɔ ka ba 'yɛrɛ, "Saa dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ a nɩtɔ̃ a Isɩral jaa ɛ."
40009034	Tɩchɛ ka a Faraseemɩne 'yɛr, "A sɩdɛbɛ nãa lɛ kʋ wʋ a kpɛ̃ɔ ka wʋ dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire."
40009035	Yesu yɔn a tẽbɛrɛ nɩ a tẽbil a jaa pɔ, wile a nɩbɛ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie pɔ, tɩ mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ sãana nɩ baal jaa bʋrɔ.
40009036	Wʋn wa nyɛ a nɩyɔɔ, nɩbaal kpɛ wʋ naa bojũu baa bɔ̃ɔ a ba ju tɩɛr ɛ, na baa mɩ lɛ tara sʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, fɩka piir na ba tara chɩnɛ ɛ.
40009037	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "A pʋɔ bɛrma naa tɩchɛ ka a ŋmaŋmarba ba waa ɛ,
40009038	a lɛ jũu yɩ sʋɔr a pʋɔ sʋɔ ka wʋ bar tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ka ba wa a pʋɔ pɔ."
40010001	Yesu bʋɔl a wʋ poturbo pie nɩ ayi na wʋ kʋ ba kpɛ̃ɔ ɩka ba dii a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi, na ba sãana nɩ baal jaa bʋrɔ.
40010002	A poturbo pie nɩ ayi na ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ yoe lɛ a anyãna, Simon ban bʋɔlɔ Pita, nɩ a wʋ yɛbɛ Andiru, Jemesɩ na ɩ Jebedee bidaba, nɩ a wʋ yɛbɛ Jɔɔn.
40010003	Filip nɩ Batolomi, Tomasɩ nɩ Matiu na ɩ a lõpodiere. Jemesɩ na ɩ Alfayasɩ bidaba nɩ Tadius.
40010004	Simon na mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a wʋ wɛr yele, nɩ Judas Isɩkariyot 'lɔ lɛ wa gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu.
40010005	A poturbo pie nɩ ayi banyã lɛ a Yesu tʋ̃ nɩ a kpãafʋ anyãna. "Yɩ ta kpɛ a nɩyor bɩɩ a Samariya tẽn pɔ ɛ,
40010006	tɩchɛ yɩ chen a Isɩral nɩbɛ bala na bɔr a piir kaar sɛ̃.
40010007	Yɩ chen tɩ mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ na yɩ 'yɛrɛ, a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ ta na.
40010008	Yɩ sãana a baalsɩ, na yɩ sɩ̃nɛ a kũusɩ, na yɩ sãana a kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ baalsɩ na yɩn maal ba ka ba ɩ nɩsʋ̃n, na yɩ dire a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire. Yɩ nyɛn pɔrɔ, yɩ mɩ tɩ tɩr pɔrɔ.
40010009	Yɩ ta de sɛlma ɛ bɩɩ diere libie 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yɩ wʋʋr pɔ ɛ,
40010010	bɩɩ 'mɔɔ wʋɔ tara a sɔr pɔ ɛ, bɩɩ 'mɔɔ fuusɩ ayi ɛ, bɩɩ de nafɔbɔ pʋ̃ɔ ɛ, bɩɩ dadiiraa ɛ, bojũu tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ jaa sɛɛn naa wʋ sãyar.
40010011	"Yɩn wa kpɛ tẽe jaa pɔ, yɩ sʋʋr kaa nɩrɛ 'lɔ nɩ na de yɩ, yɩ kpɩɛrɛ a wʋ 'yɛr na yɩ wa tɩ yɩn a be.
40010012	Yɩn wa kpɛ a yir, yɩ puor a nɩbɛ.
40010013	A yir 'lɔ nɩbɛ wa sɔɔ de yɩ, yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ nyã'maar be a ba sɛ̃, tɩchɛ bala ba wa sɔɔ de yɩ ɛ, yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ nyã'maar.
40010014	Nɩrɛ jaa baa wa sɔɔ de yɩ ɛ bɩɩ chɛl a yɩ 'yɛr ɛ, yɩ kpoor a yɩ gbɛɛ tã-uul bar yɩn wa yire be a tẽe 'lɔ bɩɩ a yir 'lɔ pɔ.
40010015	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, Nãaŋmɩn na kãan a Sodom nɩbɛ nɩ a Gomora nɩbɛ nɩbaal a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ bɩbir gar a nɩbɛ bala a tẽe 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ.
40010016	Yɩ nyɛ, n tʋ̃nɔ̃ yɩ naa fɩka piir na kpɛ jubɛrɛ pɔ kaar, yɩ ɩ yɛ̃n dẽme waba kaar, na yɩ kaara fɩka ŋmama na ba maala dɛɛr ɛ.
40010017	"Yɩ gu a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, ban nyɔɔr yɩn chiin tɩ kʋ a nɩbɛrɛ na ba fɔb yɩ a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir,
40010018	ban fɩr yɩn chiin a paal nɩbɛrɛ jie nɩ a nãmɩne yie a n yuor jũu, ka yɩ na di dãasɩɛ kʋ a bala na ɩ a nɩyor.
40010019	Ba la wa nyɔɔr yɩ chiin a 'yɛr tɔɔr fʋ jie, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a wõnõ yɩ a lɛ yɩn tɩ 'yɛrɛ ɛ nɩ a lɛ yɩn na 'yɛr ɛ; bon 'lɔ yɩn na 'yɛr Nãaŋmɩn na wiil yɩ naa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ nɔ̃.
40010020	A ba ɩ yɩn lɛ na 'yɛr ɛ tɩchɛ a yɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na wiil yɩn a lɛ yɩn na 'yɛr.
40010021	"Yɛbɛ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ yɛbɛ ka ba kʋ wʋ, ka a sãa mɩ gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ bie. Bibiir kʋ lɛ wõnõ a ba sãamɩne toor ɛ, na ba vɛ̃ ka ba kʋ ba.
40010022	Nɩrɛ jaa na 'laar yɩ naa yɩn sɔɔ ma jũu, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔɔ ara tɩ ta a baaraa, na nyɛn faafʋ.
40010023	A tẽe 'lɔ nɩbɛ wa gere yɩ, yɩ yi a be fɔɔ chen tẽyuo; yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ kʋ yɔ a Isɩral tẽn bar ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a Nɩsaal Bie wa ɛ.
40010024	"Jãjãna ba gar a wʋ wiwile ɛ bɩɩ ka gbãgbaa gar a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɛ.
40010025	A sɛɛn ɩka a jãjãna wʋ nyɛtãan a wʋ wiwile, ka a gbãgbaa mɩ nyɛtãan a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ. Ɩ ba bʋɔlɔ na a yir sʋɔ Beeljebul, yodɛɛr buor lɛ ban pãa bʋɔlɔ a yir dẽme!
40010026	"Yɩ ta joro nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, bon jaa ba be be pɔɔ ka ba kʋ̃ yuo ɛ, bɩɩ bon jaa ba be be sɔɔl ka ba kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔn ɛ.
40010027	Bon 'lɔ n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ libe pɔ yɩ 'yɛr wʋ chãa pɔ, bon 'lɔ yɩn wʋ ka ba bʋl 'yɛr yɔ̃ɔ pʋɔm 'yɛr mʋɔl wʋ a gaɩ jur.
40010028	Yɩ ta joro a bala na kʋ a ɩ̃gãn tɩ kʋ tʋ̃ɔ kʋ a sɩɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ joro a 'lɔ nɩ na tʋ̃ɔ kʋ a sɩɛ nɩ a ɩ̃gãn a bũu dagel 'lɔ pɔ.
40010029	Ba ma dãn tiitasɩ ayi kobsɩ ayi. Tɩchɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋ lo tẽe ɛ, ala baa ɩ a yɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ lɛ ɛ.
40010030	Nãaŋmɩn sɔr a yɩ jukɔɔl a jaa bɔ̃ɔ.
40010031	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, yɩ tara na tɔ̃nɔ̃ gar a tiitasɩ.
40010032	"Nɩrɛ jaa na wa 'yɛr ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔ ma naa a nɩbɛ niem, 'lɔ lɛ n mɩ na 'yɛr ɩka n bɔ̃ɔ naa a n Sãa na be a saaju niem,
40010033	tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na chiir ma a nɩbɛ niem, 'lɔ lɛ n mɩ na chiir a n Sãa na be a saaju niem.
40010034	"Yɩ ta tɩɛr ɩka nyã'maar lɛ n waan a wɛr pɔ ɛ; n ba waan nyã'maar ɛ tɩchɛ ootaa lɛ n waan.
40010035	N wan ɩka n wa vɛ̃ ka 'Bie nɩ sãa ootaa, ka bipɔɔ oo a ma, pɔɔ na oo naa a wʋ bidaba pɔɔ ka a bidaba pɔɔ mɩ oo a wʋ sɩrɛ ma.
40010036	Yir dẽme na lɩɛb ɩ dɔ̃dẽme.'
40010037	"Nɩrɛ jaa na nʋ̃ a wʋ sãa bɩɩ a wʋ ma gar ma wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a n poturo ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa mɩ na nʋ̃ a wʋ bie bɩɩ bipɔɔ gar ma, wʋ kʋ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a n poturo ɛ.
40010038	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na ba de a wʋ daa tuo turo nɩ ma ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a n poturo ɛ.
40010039	Bala na bʋɔrɔ a ba nyɛvʋr na bɔr wʋ naa tɩchɛ bala mɩ na bɔr a ba nyɛvʋr a maa jũu na nyɛ wʋ naa.
40010040	"Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de yɩ, sɔɔn de ma, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa mɩ na sɔɔ de ma sɔɔn de a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma.
40010041	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ wʋn ɩ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ jũu na nyɛn a wʋ sãyar. Nɩrɛ jaa mɩ na sɔɔ de nɩrɛ na ɩ nɩtor wʋn ɩ nɩtor jũu na nyɛn a nɩtor sãyar.
40010042	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na kʋ a bʋ̃bile banyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ kɔ̃'maar nɩ ŋmele wʋ̃n ɩ a n poturbo jũu, yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a nɩnyɩnɛ kʋ̃ faa a wʋ sãyar ɛ."
40011001	Yesu na wa wiil a wʋ poturbo pie nɩ ayi baar, wʋ yin a be chen a Juu nɩbɛ tẽn tɩ wile na wʋ mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ a tẽn ala na be a Galilee paal pɔ.
40011002	Jɔɔn na be a nɩpɔɔ die pɔ, tɩ wa wõ lɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na maala, wʋ tʋ̃n a wʋ poturbo bamɩne
40011003	ɩka ba tɩ sʋʋr, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ nɩ na wa bɩɩ, sɩ chɛlɛ nɩyuo?"
40011004	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ lɩɛb kul tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Jɔɔn, a lɛ yɩn wõ tɩ nyɛ.
40011005	Jɔ̃n nyɛrɛ naa, ka a gbɛrsɩ mɩ chiine, ka kɔ̃kɔ̃n mɩ sa, ka wõn mɩ wõnõ jaa chɛchɛ, ka kũusɩ jɛɔ, ka 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ mɩ ta a nɔ̃n dẽme.
40011006	Pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ na ba baala ma ɛ."
40011007	Ban wa chen baar, Yesu piel 'yɛrɛ a Jɔɔn 'yɛr kʋrɔ a nɩyɔɔ, "Bo lɛ yɩ dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ ɩka yɩ tɩ kaa? A jɩmur a sɛsɛbɛ na dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ bɩɩ?
40011008	Kai, ka bo lɛ yɩ chen ɩka yɩ tɩ kaa? Daba na su bʋ̃vɩɛl lɛ yɩ chen ɩka yɩ tɩ kaa bɩɩ? Nyɛ a bala na ma su bʋ̃vɩɛl ɛ, nãmɩne yie lɛ ba ma be.
40011009	Tɩchɛ bo lɛ yɩ chen ɩka yɩ tɩ kaa? Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ bɩɩ? Ɔ̃ɔ, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka wʋ gar Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ.
40011010	A nyã yele lɛ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka ɩn tʋ̃ naa a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ka wʋ de a fʋ nie na wʋ tɩ chɔɔr a fʋ sɔr kʋ fʋ.
40011011	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka bala jaa pɔɔ na dɔɔ ka a wɛr pɔ, ba ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar a Jɔɔn kɔ̃suor ɛ, tɩchɛ 'lɔ mɩ na ɩ a pʋʋr a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ gar wʋ naa.
40011012	An yi a Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suoro sɔ̃ɔ wa tɩ tãn a dɩna a Nãaŋmɩn Nãalʋ̃ʋ nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ naa ka a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme sɔ̃ɔ wʋ.
40011013	A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ba jaa nɩ a nɛbinãa dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr tɩ tãn a Jɔɔn sɔ̃ɔ.
40011014	Ala ɩ yɩn sɔɔn de, a anyãna 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Elaija nɩ naa lɩɛb wa.
40011015	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor wʋ chɛlɛ.
40011016	"Tɩchɛ bo lɛ ɩn de a dɩna nɩbɛ man? Ba nyɛntãan bibiir na ma jɩ̃nɛ a ba dɩ̃ɛn jiir na ba bʋɔlɔ taa,
40011017	sɩ pɛɛl a ɩlɛ tɩ yaa sɛɛrɛ bɩ̃nɛ ɛ, na sɩ kõnõ kõyiel yaa ŋmara nɩbikʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
40011018	A Jɔɔn na wa, waa dire ɛ, na waa lɛ nyuro go ɛ, ka ba 'yɛr ɩka sɩdɛɛr lɛ wʋ ɩ.
40011019	Tɩchɛ ka a Nɩsaal Bie wa na wʋ ma dire tɩ nyuro ka ba 'yɛr ɩka di dire nɩ dãburo lɛ wʋ ɩ, na wʋ ɩ a lõpodierbe nɩ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ baraa. A ma wiil a lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na tor, bala wa nyɛ lɛ a wʋ nɩbɛ na kpɩɛrɛ nɩ yɛ̃."
40011020	Yesu pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔn naa a tẽn bala nɩbɛ a be a wʋ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ na tʋ̃, tɩchɛ ka baa sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ.
40011021	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn Korajin dẽme sɛ̃. Nɛbier mɩ ben a yɩn Betɩsaida dẽme sɛ̃. A a ɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala ɩn tʋ̃ a yɩ jie, mɩ ta tʋ̃n be a lɛ a Tire nɩ a Sidon tẽn pɔ, ban taa lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr na ba su bʋ̃jarsɩ jɛn tãpɩɛl pɔ.
40011022	Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar Nãaŋmɩn na kãan a Tire nɩ a Sidon nɩbɛ nɩbaal gar a yɩn.
40011023	A yɩn Kapenahum dẽme, ban 'mɔɔ yɩn don saaju bɩɩ? Kai, ban suun yɩn a kpĩisɩ tẽe. Ala ɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ na tʋ̃ a yɩ pɔ mɩ ta tʋ̃n a Sodom pɔ, a tẽe anyãna naa chɛnɛ na wa tɔ dɩna.
40011024	Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar Nãaŋmɩn na kãan Sodom nɩbɛ nɩbaal gar a yɩn."
40011025	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ Yesu 'yɛr naa, "N dãn a n Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a saaju nɩ a tẽe wʋ jaa Soro, bojũu fʋ sɔɔl a yele anyãna a yɛ̃n dẽme sɛ̃ tɩ ir wiil bibiir.
40011026	Ɔ̃ɔ, n Sãa lɛ lɛ ɩ a fʋ pʋpɛl ka fʋ maal.
40011027	"N Sãa den a yele a jaa kʋ, nɩrɛ jaa ba bɔ̃ɔ a Bie ɛ, ka a Sãa ba lɛ ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa mɩ ba bɔ̃ɔ a Sãa ɛ, ka a Bie ba lɛ ɛ, nɩ a bala a Nãaŋmɩn Bie na ir, na wiil ban a Sãa.
40011028	"Yɩ wa a n sɛ̃, yɩn banyã na bal na yɩ tuo tuor ka a wõnõ yɩ, ɩn too yɩn a yɩ pɛ̃n.
40011029	Yɩ de a n daa tuo na yɩ jãn yi a n sɛ̃, bojũu n ɩn jomm sʋɔ, naa siir a n mɩ̃ɛ a n nyãa pɔ, yɩn nyɛn pɛ̃nfʋ kʋ a yɩ sɩɩr.
40011030	Bojũu a n daa ɩn kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃, ka yɩn tʋ̃ɔ tuo a tuor ala ɩn na kʋ yɩ."
40012001	A ba kor ɛ tɩchɛ ka Yesu kpɛ a pʋɔ sãlsɔɔ tala a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar. Kɔ̃ kpɛ̃n a wʋ poturbo, ka ba piel fɔrɔ a bʋ̃bie ɔɔrɔ.
40012002	A Faraseemɩne na wa nyɛ a lɛ, ba sʋʋr a Yesu, "Fʋ nyɛn lɛ na ba tu a nɛbinãa a fʋ poturbo na ɩrɛ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar ɔ?"
40012003	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yaa kar a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ nyɛ a lɛ a Nãa David na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ a kɔ̃ na kpɛ ɛ?
40012004	Wʋ kpɛ̃n a Nãaŋmɩn yir ka 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ tɩ de a paanʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban ben kʋ Nãaŋmɩn na ba 'wɔb na ba tara sɔr ɛ, ka ala ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrloro tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
40012005	Bɩɩ yaa kar a Mosesɩ nɛbinãa pɔ lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlorbo a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar a puorfʋ yir pɔ na ma tʋ̃ tɩ na baa bʋɔlɔ a lɛ bier ɛ?
40012006	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ ben ka na gar a puorfʋ yir.
40012007	A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr a, 'Nɩbaal lɛ n bʋɔrɔ, a ba ɩ dʋ̃n yɩn kʋ chʋm kʋ ma ɛ.' Yɩn ta bɔ̃ɔ a yele nyã par, yɩ kʋ naa bʋɔlɔ nɩbɛ na ba maal dɛɛr ɛ, ɩka bier lɛ ba maal ɛ.
40012008	A maa Nɩsaal Bie lɛ ɩ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Soro."
40012009	Yesu yin a be chen a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir pɔ,
40012010	tɩ nyɛ daba kɔ̃ɔ nũu na kpi. Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "A tara na sɔr ɩka fʋ sãa baal a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar ɔ?" Ba sʋʋr a lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba nyɛ a wʋ pɔ 'yɛr 'yɛr.
40012011	Yesu sʋʋr naa, "Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ tara na pɛr ka wʋ lo bulo pɔ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar, ŋmɛ lɛ fʋn ɩ? A ba ɩ fʋn ir wʋn a bɔɔ pɔ ɛ?
40012012	A nɩsaal gar pɛr. A lɛ jũu a sɩ nɛbinãa bar sɔr ɩka fʋ maal vɩla kʋ nɩrɛ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar."
40012013	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba 'lɔ nũu na kpi, "Tur a fʋ nũu." A wʋ tur ka a nũu wʋ jaa sa kaara a nũu nyã sʋɔ kaar.
40012014	A Faraseemɩne yin na ba piel guoro a Yesu kʋfʋ.
40012015	Yesu na wa bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban piel guoro ɩka ba ɩ wʋ, wʋ yin a jie 'lɔ ka nɩyɔɔ jaa turo wʋ. Wʋ sãan a bala an ɔɔrɔ.
40012016	Tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba ɩka ba ta 'yɛr a wʋ yele kʋ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ.
40012017	Wʋ maal a nɩtɔ̃, ka a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr tu a 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Isaiya na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ,
40012018	"A n tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a nyã ɩn kaa ir, a 'lɔ n na nʋ̃, a 'lɔ a n pʋɔ na pɛlʋ. Ɩn yɔ̃ɔ wʋn a n Sɩɛ, ka wʋ mʋɔl a n 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ yele kʋ a nɩbɛ ba jaa.
40012019	Wʋ kʋ tara nɛchɩrɛ bɩɩ ŋmiere chɛlsɩ bɩɩ pɔɔrɔ gɔ̃mɔ̃ yõo ɛ.
40012020	Wʋn siir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a bala na siir a ba mɩ̃ɛ, tɩ na wʋ maal vɩla kʋ a bala na ba tara sʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ. Wʋn ara na kpɛ̃ɔ tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn na vɛ̃ ka a nɩbɛ sɔɔ de a Nãaŋmɩn yeltorsɩ.
40012021	A wʋ yuor pɔ lɛ a nɩbɛ ba jaa na tara tɩɛrtɔ fʋ jie."
40012022	Ba waan na daba na ɩ jɔ̃ɔ tɩ ɩ wõo na tara sɩdɛbɛ Yesu sɛ̃. Wʋ sãn a daba baal, ka wʋ nyɛrɛ tɩ lɛ 'yɛrɛ jaa chɛchɛ.
40012023	Nɛɛr 'maan a nɩyɔɔ ka ba sʋrɔ taa ɩka, kaa 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nãa David Bie bɩɩ?
40012024	Tɩchɛ a Faraseemɩne na wa wõ a lɛ ba 'yɛr naa, "Wʋ dire na sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire bojũu, a sɩdɛbɛ nãa Beeljebul lɛ kʋ wʋ a kpɛ̃ɔ ka wʋ dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ."
40012025	Yesu na bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban tɩɛrɛ, a wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Tẽe 'lɔ na ŋma dẽdẽme jɛɛrɛ taa kʋ kor ɛ. Tẽe 'lɔ bɩɩ yir kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ na ŋma dẽdẽme jɛɛrɛ taa kʋ ara ɛ.
40012026	Ala ɩ a Satan diin Satan kʋ yi na wʋ ŋma dẽdẽme ŋmɛ lɛ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ na ɩ ara?
40012027	Ala ɩ Beeljebul lɛ kʋ ma a kpɛ̃ɔ ka dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ, tɩ a bala na ɩ a yɩ poturbo, bo lɛ ba tara dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ? A lɛ jũu bala lɛ na ɩ a yɩ 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ.
40012028	Ala ɩ Satan diin Satan kʋ yi na wʋ ŋma dẽdẽme ŋmɛ lɛ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ na ɩ ara? Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ lɛ kʋ ma a kpɛ̃ɔ ka dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire wiil ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ ta yɩ naa.
40012029	"Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ nɩrɛ na tʋ̃ɔ ɩ kar kpɛ gãdaa yir de a wʋ bonsɩ, 'lɔ ba de nie lũ a gãdaa nyã tɩ de a wʋ bonsɩ ɛ?
40012030	"Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba be a n sɛ̃ ɛ, tara man nɩ 'yɛr, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba pʋɔ ma a sɩ kaal lɔ̃ɔ taa ɛ wʋ ma yɛ̃yɛl bar.
40012031	A lɛ jũu n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka nɩbɛ na nyɛn yelbier jaa nɩ 'yɛrdɛɛr jaa ban 'yɛr vɛ̃ kʋ fʋ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋ nyɛ yelbier vɛ̃ kʋ fʋ ɛ.
40012032	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na nyɛn yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋ nyɛ yelbier vɛ̃ kʋ fʋ ɛ. Dɩna nɩ daar kɔ̃ɔ.
40012033	"Ala ɩ tɩɛ vɩɛlɛ na wʋ ma wɔ̃n wɔ̃vɩɛl, ala ɩ tɩɛ ɩn tɩdɛɛr wʋ ma wɔ̃n wɔ̃dɛbɛ. Tɩɛ jaa a wʋ wɔ̃mɔ̃ lɛ ba ma de bɔ̃ɔn wʋ.
40012034	Yɩn waa bibiir! Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩn tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr 'yɛr vɩɛlsɩ ala ɩ yɩ ɩn yelbe-ɩrbɛ? A ala na sɛɛ a pʋɔ lɛ a nɛɛ ma 'yɛr.
40012035	A nɩsʋ̃ a yelsʋ̃n ala na be a wʋ pʋɔm lɛ wʋ ma 'yɛr, ka a nɩdɛɛr mɩ ma 'yɛr a yeldɛbɛ ala na be a wʋ pʋɔm.
40012036	Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar, nɩrɛ jaa na man 'yɛrdɛɛr 'lɔ jaa bʋrɔ na dɔ̃ɔ yi a wʋ nɛɛ pɔ.
40012037	A fʋ 'yɛrbie lɛ na wiil a lɛ fʋn be, naa wiil a fʋ sɔ̃ɔnaa."
40012038	Be lɛ ka a nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne bamɩne 'yɛr, "Wiwile, sɩ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka sɩ nyɛ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ na ɩ jɩ̃nɛ a fʋ jie."
40012039	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A yɩn banyãna na ɩ a putudẽme nɩ sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ tɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n tʋ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ka a na ɩ jɩ̃nɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Jona jɩ̃nɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
40012040	Nɩtãa lɛ a Jona na dɔ̃ɔ gã a jɩ̃nele pʋɔm ber ata nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ gbulo ata lɛ mɩ lɛ a Maa Nɩsaal Bie mɩ na gã a yaa pɔ ber ata nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ gbulo ata.
40012041	A 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar Ninive nɩbɛ na yin 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ 'yɛr, bojũu ba lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr a Jona na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ ba, tɩchɛ yɩ kaa, a 'lɔ na gar a Jona ben ka.
40012042	A pɔɔ nãa na yin be a par a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar na wʋ wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ 'yɛr, bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ yi be a tẽtɛɛr wa chɛl a Nãa Solomon yɛ̃ 'yɛr, tɩchɛ yɩ kaa a 'lɔ na gar a Solomon ben ka.
40012043	"Sɩdɛɛr wa yɩ nɩrɛ pɔ, wʋ ma chen dãlpʋʋr pɔ tɩ bʋɔrɔ pɛ̃nfʋ jie 'lɔ baa wa nyɛ ɛ,
40012044	wʋ ma 'yɛr naa ɩn lɩɛb kul a yir 'lɔ pɔ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ yɩ. Wʋ wa nyɛn a yir ka wʋ ɩ yirkpolo na wʋ vɩɛlɛ,
40012045	ka wʋ chen tɩ bʋɔl sɩdɛbɛ ayopõi na tara a putuo gar wʋ ka ba tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a be. Ka a nɩrɛ nyã pãa ɩ dɛɛr gar a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ be. Lɛ lɛ an kaara a yɩn putudẽme a dɩna."
40012046	Wʋn chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ nɩ a nɩyɔɔ, a wʋ ma nɩ a wʋ yɛɛr wa ben yõo bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba nyɛ wʋ.
40012047	Nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Nyɛ a fʋ ma nɩ a fʋ yɛɛr lɛ be yõo bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba nyɛ fʋ."
40012048	Tɩchɛ Yesu sʋʋr a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'yɛr a 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "An lɛ a ɩ ma nɩ ba boo lɛ ɩ a n yɛɛr?"
40012049	Wʋ lɩɛb tur a wʋ poturbo nũu tɩ 'yɛr, "Nyɛ a n ma nɩ a n yɛɛr!
40012050	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na maala a lɛ a n Sãa na be a saaju na bʋɔrɔ lɛ ɩ a n yɛɛr nɩ a n ma."
40013001	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ Yesu yin a yir pɔ tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a man kõkoor.
40013002	A nɩyɔɔ na lɔ̃ɔ jũu wʋ kpɛ̃n jɛ̃ a gboro pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a nɩyɔɔ ara a man kõkoor.
40013003	Sʋkpar lɛ wʋ lɔɔrɔ wile nɩ ba yelyɔɔ, "Yɩ chɛlɛ, kʋɔraa lɛ yin wʋ bʋ̃bʋrɔ bʋrfʋ jie.
40013004	Wʋ tɩ yaara na yʋɔrɔ nɩ ka amɩne lo sɔr pɔ, ka lubil tuur di.
40013005	A bʋ̃bie amɩne mɩ lon kʋsɩr pãn ju naa bul tɩ kpi bojũu tãn ba waa ɛ.
40013006	Tɩchɛ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa nyãa, a bʋ̃bulo jʋɔl naa kpi, bojũu a ba ba nyɩbɛ ɛ.
40013007	Ka amɩne mɩ lo gʋʋr pɔ 'mataa bul ka a gʋʋr nʋ̃ɔ fɩ̃ɩn ba.
40013008	Tɩchɛ amɩne mɩ lon kɔjɔ̃ pɔ bul dɔɔ jur kɔbaa, amɩne lɩjaata amɩne lɩjɛr nɩ pie.
40013009	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor wʋ chɛlɛ."
40013010	A poturbo wan a wʋ sɛ̃ wa sʋʋr, "Bo lɛ so fʋn ma lɔɔrɔ a sʋkpar kʋrɔ ba?"
40013011	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn 'lɔ ɩn vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ yelsɔɔlsɩ tɩchɛ a bala na chɛ sʋkpar lɛ n lɔɔrɔ kʋrɔ ba.
40013012	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na tara Nãaŋmɩn tɩɛr, Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃n ka a nɩnyɩnɛ bɔ̃ɔfʋ pʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ, tɩchɛ a bala jaa na ba bʋɔrɔ a wʋ bɔ̃ɔfʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn na pɔɔn a ba tɩɛr.
40013013	A par nɩ nyã ɩn lɔɔrɔ a sʋkpar kʋrɔ ba, ba ma kaa naa tɩ maa nyɛ ɛ, na ba ma wõ tɩ maa bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ.
40013014	Bala 'lɔ an ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Isaiya na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩka, 'A nɩbɛ banyã na ma wõ naa tɩ ba kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, ban ma kaa naa tɩ ba kʋ̃ nyɛ ɛ.
40013015	A nɩbɛ banyã nyãn dar naa ka a ba tobo pɔɔ baa wõnõ ɛ, na ba ũu a ba nɩbie, ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, ban taa kãan naa a ba nɩbie na ba wõn a ba tobo, na ba bɔ̃ɔ a par, na ba lɩɛb wa ka n sãa ba.'
40013016	Tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ, yɩ ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n dẽme, a yɩ nɩbie na nyɛ, ka a yɩ tobo mɩ wõ.
40013017	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ yɔɔ nɩ nɩtorsɩ yɔɔ ta bʋɔrɔ na ɩka ba nyɛ bon 'lɔ yɩn nyɛ tɩchɛ baa nyɛ ɛ, na ba ta wõ bon 'lɔ yɩn wõ tɩchɛ baa tʋ̃ɔ wõ ɛ.
40013018	"Yɩ pãa chɛlɛ a kʋɔraa sʋkpa par,
40013019	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na wõ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr tɩ ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, a dɛɛr sʋɔ ma wan wa ir a bon 'lɔ na bʋr a wʋ nyãa pɔ, a bʋ̃bie anyã lɛ, a ala na lo a sɔr pɔ.
40013020	Ala mɩ na lo a kʋsɩr pãn ju lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na wõ a 'yɛr sɔɔ de fɔfɔɔ jaa nɩ pʋpɛl,
40013021	tɩchɛ a nɩrɛ nyã ba ba nyɩbɛ ɛ, na wʋ di kãnyir ara bɩ̃lãa, a lɛ jũu wõm bɩɩ bɛɛr kaa wa pɔɔ wʋ a 'yɛr jũu, a nɩrɛ nyã ma lo naa.
40013022	A bʋ̃bie ala mɩ na lo a gʋʋr pɔ, 'lɔ lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na wõ a 'yɛr tɩ nʋ̃ a wɛr ju nyɛvʋr yelwõnsɩ nɩ a wɛr ju bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ fɩ̃ɩn a 'yɛr ka waa dɔɔ bie ɛ.
40013023	Tɩchɛ a bʋ̃bie ala na lo a kɔjɔ̃ pɔ lɛ a nɩrɛ nyã na wõ a 'yɛr bɔ̃ɔ a par, 'lɔ lɛ wɔ̃ wɔ̃mɔ̃ dɔɔ jur, amɩne kɔbaa, amɩne lɩjaata amɩne mɩ lɩjɛr nɩ pie."
40013024	Yesu lɛ lɔb a sʋkpa ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋ ba, "Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ ɩn de a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ man. Nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ bʋr bʋ̃bivɩɛl a wʋ pʋɔ pɔ,
40013025	nɩrɛ jaa na wa gã gur baar, a dɔ̃sʋɔ wan wa bʋr mɔɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a chi pɔ tɩ na wʋ kul.
40013026	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a chi na wa tɩ bulo ka a mɔɩ mɩ bul puro.
40013027	"A daba tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ wan wa sʋʋr wʋ, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, a ba ɩ bʋ̃bivɩɛl lɛ fʋ bʋr a pʋɔ pɔ ɛ; tɩ nyɛ a mɔɩ mɩ yi?'
40013028	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Dɔ̃sʋɔ lɛ tʋ̃ a lɛ.' A tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ sʋʋr wʋ, 'Fʋ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka sɩ chen tɩ vɔ̃ a mɔɩ bar bɩɩ?'
40013029	"Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Kai, yɩn be vɔ̃nɔ̃ a mɔɩ, yɩn wa vɔ̃n a chi mɩ bar.
40013030	Yɩ bar ka a 'mataa nʋ̃ɔ tɩ tãn a ŋmafʋ daar, ɩn 'yɛr kʋ a ŋmaŋmarba ka ba dɔ̃ɔ vɔ̃ a mɔɩ lũ lũ chʋm bar tɩ ŋma a chi 'yɔ̃ɔ a n boor pɔ.' "
40013031	Yesu lɛ lɔb a sʋkpa ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋ ba go, "A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ kaara naa fɩka kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ bir nɩrɛ na de bʋr a wʋ pʋɔ pɔ.
40013032	'Lɔ lɛ a bʋ̃bie a jaa pɔ bʋ̃bile tɩchɛ 'lɔ wa nʋ̃ɔ, 'lɔ lɛ ma ɩ a tɩɩr a jaa pɔ tɩkpɛ̃ɛ, ka lubil ma 'yɔ̃ɔ choor a wʋ ju."
40013033	Wʋ lɛ lɔb a sʋkpa ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋ ba, "A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ kaara naa fɩka dãbɩl pɔɔ na de 'yɔ̃ɔ jɔ̃ yɔɔ pɔ ka a ir vʋ̃."
40013034	Yesu den sʋkpar 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩ a nɩyɔɔ a yelsɩ anyã, wʋ maa 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ ba ka waa lɔb sʋkpa ɛ.
40013035	A nyã lɛ na wiil ɩka a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ, "Ɩka ɩn ma den a n nɛɛ lɔɔrɔ nɩ sʋkpar naa wiil yɩ yelsɩ ala na sɔɔl a wɛr pielfʋ daar."
40013036	Wʋ yin a nɩyɔɔ pɔ kpɛ a yir, ka a wʋ poturbo wa a wʋ sɛ̃ wa 'yɛrɛ, wiil sɩ a mɔɩ na be a pʋɔ pɔ sʋkpa par.
40013037	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bʋr a bʋ̃bivɩɛl lɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie.
40013038	A pʋɔ lɛ ɩ a wɛr. A bʋ̃bivɩɛl lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ bibiir. A mɔɩ lɛ a bala na ɩ a dɛɛr sʋɔ bibiir.
40013039	A dɔ̃sʋɔ 'lɔ mɩ na bʋr lɛ ɩ a tɩɩ. A ŋmafʋ lɛ ɩ a wɛr baarfʋ daar, a ŋmaŋmarba lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn malakasɩ.
40013040	"Lɛ ban na chʋm a mɔɩ bũu pɔ ka a di, lɛ mɩ lɛ na ɩ a wɛr baarfʋ daar.
40013041	A maa Nɩsaal Bie na tʋ̃n a n malakasɩ ka ba wa tuur a nɩsʋ̃n a nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ, tɩchɛ a bala jaa na vɛ̃ ka a nɩbɛ maala yelbier nɩ yelbe-ɩrbɛ ba jaa 'mataa bar.
40013042	Ka ba lɔb ba 'yɔ̃ɔ bũu dagel pɔ, be lɛ ban kõnõ ɔɔrɔ nɩ nyɩmɛ.
40013043	A bala na tor na chaar naa mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ kaar a ba Sãa nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara tobo wʋ chɛlɛ.
40013044	"A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ kaara naa fɩka nɩrɛ na nyɛ nãbonsɩ pʋɔ pɔ 'mɔɔ sɔɔl tɩchɛ ka a wʋ pʋɔ pɛl, ka wʋ tɩ da a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa wʋn tara tɩ dãn a puo.
40013045	"A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ lɛ kaara naa fɩka nɩrɛ na yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ kʋsɩvɩɛl,
40013046	wʋn wa nyɛ a ɩ̃sʋɔ daa na be tuo, wʋ tɩ dãn a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa tɩ dãn.
40013047	"A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ lɛ nyɛntãan fɩka lɔyaar ban lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ man pɔ, kʋ nyɔɔr jɩ̃dẽdẽme.
40013048	A lɔyaar na wa sɛɛ ba tɔɔn yin a gogoro ju, tɩ jɩ̃nɛ tuur a jɩ̃sʋ̃n 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɛr pɔ, tɩ lɔb a jɩ̃dɛbɛ bar.
40013049	Lɛ lɛ an be a wɛr baarfʋ daar. A Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃n a wʋ malakasɩ ka ba wa tuur a nɩdɛbɛ yin a nɩmɩn pɔ,
40013050	tɩ na ba lɔb a nɩdɛbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a bũu dagel pɔ, be lɛ ban kõnõ tɩ ɔɔrɔ nyɩmɛ.
40013051	"Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a yelsɩ anyã na a jaa par ɔ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ."
40013052	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A nɛɛ wile ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ban wiil ka wʋ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ yele kaara naa fɩka yir sʋɔ na de bʋ̃paalaa nɩ bʋ̃koro yin a wʋ boor pɔ."
40013053	Yesu na wa wiil a sʋkpar anyã par, wʋ yin a be.
40013054	Wʋ wan a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ paal pɔ tɩ piel wile a nɩbɛ a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir, ka nɛɛr 'maa ba ka ba 'yɛr, "Nyɛ lɛ a daba nyã nyɛ a yɛ̃ nyã nɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ a nyã?
40013055	A ba ɩ a mɩmɩɛrɛ bidaba lɛ ɛ? A ba ɩ a wʋ ma lɛ ba bʋɔlɔ a Mɛɛr ɛ? A ba ɩ a wʋ yɛɛr nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ Josefʋ nɩ Simon nɩ Judas ɛ?
40013056	A ba ɩ sɩn nɩ a wʋ yɛpɔbɔ ba jaa lɛ 'mataa be a ka ɛ? Nyɩnɛ lɛ a daba nyã nyɛ a kpɛ̃ɔ nyã?"
40013057	Tɩ na ba tɔr a wʋ yele. Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ nyɛrɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ jie jaa tɩchɛ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tẽe nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yir pɔ, wʋ maa nyɛ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ ɛ."
40013058	Ban ba sɔɔ de wʋ jũu, waa tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃yɔɔ a be ɛ.
40014001	A ber ala pɔ, a Hɛrɔd na ɩ a Galilee nãa wõn a Yesu yele
40014002	na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ, "Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suor lɛ tɔ̃ɔ ir ɩ vʋr, ala lɛ so ka wʋ tara a kpɛ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ anyãna."
40014003	A Nãa Hɛrɔd vɛ̃n ka ba nyɔɔ Jɔɔn lũ 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩpɔɔ die pɔ a wʋ yɛbɛ Filip pɔɔ Hɛrɔdiyas jũu.
40014004	Bojũu Jɔɔn ma 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ wʋ ɩka, "A ba tara sɔr ka fʋ kul wʋ ɛ."
40014005	Hɛrɔd ta bʋɔrɔ na a wʋ kʋ fʋ tɩ joro a Juu nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ bojũu ba sɔɔn ɩka wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ.
40014006	A Hɛrɔd dɔɔfʋ bɩbir dɩ̃ɛn daar, a Hɛrɔdiyas bipɔɔ sɛn bɩ̃nɛ a nɩyɔɔ niem, ka a Hɛrɔd pʋɔ pɛl
40014007	yɔɔ jaa ka wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ nɛɛ kʋ a pɔɔbile, "Sʋɔr ma bon jaa fʋn bʋɔrɔ ɩn kʋ fʋ naa."
40014008	A wʋ ma wiil wʋn a bon 'lɔ wʋn na sʋɔr, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "N bʋɔrɔ na ɩka fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suor ju a la'yɛlma pɔ kʋ ma a pʋ̃pãanyãna."
40014009	A nãa pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa, tɩchɛ wʋn faa 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɛɛ a nɩyɔɔ niem ɩka a lɛ a pɔɔbile na bʋɔrɔ a ɩ.
40014010	Wʋ tʋ̃n ka ba ŋmaa a Jɔɔn ju a nɩpɔɔ die pɔ.
40014011	Ba 'yɔ̃ɔn a ju a la'yɛlma pɔ wa kʋ a pɔɔbile, ka wʋ de kʋ a wʋ ma.
40014012	Jɔɔn poturbo wan wa 'mɔɔ a ɩ̃gãn tɩ ũu tɩ na ba tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu.
40014013	A Yesu na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃, wʋ kpɛ̃n a gboro chen jiyuo 'lɔ wʋ yõ. Tɩchɛ a nɩyɔɔ na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃ ba yin a tẽn ala pɔ bɩɛr wʋ nɩ gbɛɛ chen a be.
40014014	Wʋn wa yi a gboro pɔ, wʋ nyɛn nɩyɔɔ ka nɩbaal kpɛ wʋ tɩchɛ ka wʋ sãa a ba baalsɩ.
40014015	Mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa mʋrɔ, a poturbo wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A ka ɩn mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ ka a sɔ̃ɔ mɩ po, bar a nɩbɛ sɔr ka ba chen a tẽbil pɔ, tɩ da bʋ̃diir di."
40014016	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A ba sɛɛ ɩka ba chen ɛ, yɩ kʋ ba bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ ka ba di."
40014017	Ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu nɩ jɩ̃mɛ ayi tɛɛ lɛ sɩ tara."
40014018	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ de wa kʋ ma."
40014019	Wʋ vɛ̃n ka a nɩyɔɔ banyãna jɛ̃ tẽe. Wʋ den a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu nɩ a jɩ̃mɛ ayi ala dʋl kaa saaju tɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan tɩ na wʋ ŋma de kʋ a poturbo ɩka ba de põ a nɩbɛ. Ka a poturbo de põ a nɩbɛ.
40014020	Ba jaa din tɩɩ tɩchɛ ka a poturbo wob a bʋ̃ŋmaarsɩ ala na chɛ sɛɛ pɛr pie nɩ ayi.
40014021	A bala na di tɩɩ tɛɛ ɩn dɔɔr tur anũu ka pɔbɔ nɩ bibiir ba pʋɔ ɛ.
40014022	Ajienaa lɛ, wʋ vɛ̃n ka a poturbo kpɛ a gboro gɔ̃ɔ a man gɔ̃ɔn tɩchɛ ka wʋ vɛ̃ ka a nɩbɛ yaar.
40014023	Wʋn wa wɛl a nɩbɛ baar, wʋ don a tɔ̃ɔ ju ɩka wʋ tɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn. Jãanʋɔr na wa ta, wʋ chɛnɛ na be a be a wʋ yõ.
40014024	Tɩchɛ a kɔ̃sɛbɛ ŋmen a gboro dãdaal chiin tɛɛr ka wʋ jãan a man nɛɛ, bojũu a kɔ̃sɛbɛ fɔ̃ɔ gar ba naa.
40014025	A wɛr na wa chaara wa la la la ba nyɛn a Yesu na chiine a kʋ̃ɔ ju waara a ba sɛ̃.
40014026	A poturbo na wa nyɛ a Yesu na chiine a kʋ̃ɔ ju waara a ba sɛ̃, dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba naa, ka ba kõ 'yɛr, "Kpĩin lɛ!"
40014027	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ tara kãnyir, maa lɛ, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ."
40014028	Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N Soro, ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka chiine a kʋ̃ɔ ju wa a fʋ sɛ̃."
40014029	Ka wʋ 'yɛr wʋ, "Wa," ka Pita yi a gboro pɔ piel chiine a kʋ̃ɔ ju waara a Yesu sɛ̃.
40014030	Pita na nyɛ a sɛsɛbɛ na furo yɔɔ dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ wʋ naa, ka wʋ piel mʋrɔ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ, ka wʋ bʋɔl, "N Soro, faa ma."
40014031	Ajienaa lɛ, a Yesu tur a wʋ nũu nyɔɔ wʋ tɩ 'yɛr, "Fʋ̃ʋ sɔɔfʋ na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ, bo so ka fʋ baala?"
40014032	Ban wa kpɛ a gboro pɔ baar ka a sɛsɛbɛ ŋmaa jaa jomm.
40014033	A bala na be a gboro pɔ gbur dumo puor wʋ tɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie."
40014034	Ban wa gɔ̃ɔ a man baar ba chen a Genesaretɩ wɛr pɔ.
40014035	A tẽe 'lɔ dẽme na wa wõ a wʋ yele ba 'yɛr lʋɔr a paal 'lɔ wʋ jaa na ba waan bala jaa an ɔɔrɔ,
40014036	na ba wa sʋɔrɔ ɩka ba sɩɩr a wʋ fuu nɛɛ, a bala jaa na sɩɩr a fuu nɛɛ sa naa.
40015001	A Faraseemɩne nɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe bamɩne na yi a Jerusalɛm wan a Yesu sɛ̃ wa sʋʋr wʋ,
40015002	"Ŋmɩnɛ a fʋ poturbo ba turo a sɩ sãakpãmɩne wiilfʋ ɛ? Ba maa pɛɛ a ba nuur tɩ di ɛ."
40015003	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ ka yɩ sɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛbinsɩ tɩ na yɩ turo a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ wiilfʋ?
40015004	Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa, ''Yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ sãa nɩ a fʋ ma,' ka 'Nɩrɛ jaa wa pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ sãa bɩɩ a wʋ ma, ba kʋ wʋ.'
40015005	Tɩchɛ yɩn 'yɛr ɩka nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na 'yɛr a wʋ sãa bɩɩ ma ɩka, sʋ̃ʋfʋ 'lɔ jaa ɩn tara naa kʋ fʋ, n den kʋ Nãaŋmɩn.
40015006	Tɩchɛ na waa de a wʋ bʋ̃tarsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a a wʋ sãa ɛ, yɩn ɩ a lɛ, yɩ sɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ, tɩ na yɩ turo a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ binfʋ.
40015007	Yɩn nɛɛr ayi dẽme! Isaiya 'yɛr yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩka,
40015008	'A nɩbɛ banyãna den a ba nɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ ma tɩchɛ a ba nyãn pɔ, ba tɔɔn jãan ma.
40015009	A ba puorfʋ ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ ma ɛ, nɩsaal wiilfʋ lɛ ba wile.' "
40015010	Yesu bʋɔl a nɩyɔɔ a ba wa a wʋ sɛ̃, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chɛlɛ na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a par.
40015011	A ba ɩ bon 'lɔ na ma tu a nɩsaal nɛɛ pɔ kpɛ lɛ ma sɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ bon 'lɔ na ma yɩ a nɩsaal nɛɛ pɔ lɛ ma sɔ̃ɔ wʋ."
40015012	A poturbo wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Fʋ bɔ̃ɔn naa an kpɛ a Faraseemɩne ban wõ a 'yɛr nyã fʋn 'yɛr ɔ?"
40015013	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Tɩɛ 'lɔ jaa a n Sãa na be a saaju na ba sɛl ɛ, ɩn vʋ̃ɔ wʋn bar.
40015014	Yɩ bar ba, jɔ̃n lɛ tɔɔrɔ jɔ̃n. Jɔ̃ɔ wa tɔɔrɔ a wʋ jɔ̃ɔ tɔ sʋɔ ba jaa ma lon bɔɔ pɔ."
40015015	Tɩchɛ ka Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wiil a sʋkpa nyã par kʋ sɩ."
40015016	Be lɛ wʋ 'yɛr, "A yɩn mɩ na ɩ a n poturbo ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ?
40015017	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ka bon 'lɔ jaa na tu a nɛɛ pɔ kpɛ a pʋɔ pɔ ma tun a par bɔɔ pɔ yi bɩɩ?
40015018	Tɩchɛ bon 'lɔ na ma yi a nɛɛ pɔ, yin a tɩɛr pɔ, anyãna lɛ ma sɔ̃ɔ a nɩsaal.
40015019	A nɩsaal tɩɛr pɔ lɛ a tɩɛr dɛbɛ ma yi, nɩrɛ kʋfʋ, pɔɔdeyele, sɛ̃sɛ̃yele, nãnyiyele, jir dãasɩɛ, nɩ a gagaryele ma be.
40015020	A anyãna lɛ a bonsɩ ala na ma sɔ̃ɔ a nɩsaal tɩchɛ nɩrɛ na din nũdɛbɛ ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ ɛ."
40015021	Yesu yin a be chen a Tire paal nɩ Sidon paal pɔ.
40015022	Be lɛ a pɔɔ na yi a Kanaan paal pɔ yi piel ŋmiere chɛlsɩ, "N Soro kaa a n nɩbaal David Bie, a sɩdɛɛr lɛ tara a n bipɔɔ."
40015023	Tɩchɛ a Yesu ba 'yɛr 'yɛr jaa kʋ wʋ ɛ. Ka a wʋ poturbo wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Dii wʋ bar, wʋ pɔɔrɔ sɩn gɔ̃mɔ̃."
40015024	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "A piir ala na bɔr a Isɩral nɩbɛ pɔ tɛɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ ba tʋ̃ ma."
40015025	Tɩchɛ ka a pɔɔ wa gbur dumo a wʋ niem 'yɛr, "N Soro, sʋ̃ʋ ma."
40015026	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "A ba sɛɛ ɩka fʋ de bibiir bʋ̃diir lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ baar ɛ."
40015027	Ka a pɔɔ 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, n Soro, a baar gba ma dire na a bʋ̃di pʋr pʋr ala na ma ŋmara loro a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ dakɔɔ pĩlem."
40015028	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a pɔɔ, "Pɔɔ, a fʋ sɔɔfʋ bɛrma naa! A ɩ kʋ fʋ a lɛ fʋn bʋɔrɔ." A wʋ bipɔɔ sa naa a dẽdẽe daa 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
40015029	Yesu na wa yi a be, wʋ den a Galilee man yal kõkoor 'lana, na wʋ tɩ do tɔ̃ɔ ju jɩ̃nɛ.
40015030	A nɩyɔɔ tara na a nɩbɛ gbɛɛ na kpi kpi, nɩ jɔ̃n, nɩ a gbɛrsɩ, nɩ a wõn 'matãan baalsɩ yɔɔ waan a wʋ sɛ̃. Ba wa bin ban a wʋ niem a wʋ sãa a ba jaa baalsɩ.
40015031	Nɛɛr 'maan a nɩbɛ ban wõ ka a wõn 'yɛrɛ, ka a gbɛrsɩ sa chiine ka a bala a gbɛɛ nɩ na kpi kpi mɩ sa ka a jɔ̃n mɩ nyɛrɛ. Ka ba dãna a Isɩral nɩbɛ Nãaŋmɩn.
40015032	Yesu bʋɔl a wʋ poturbo wa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩbaal kpɛ ma naa nɩ a nɩyɔɔ banyãna bojũu ba ben a n sɛ̃ ber ata tɩ ba di bon jaa ɛ, n ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka n vɛ̃ ka ba lɩɛb chiine kɔ̃ ɛ, amɩne ban wa lon sɔr pɔ."
40015033	Ka a wʋ poturbo 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Nyɛ lɛ sɩn nyɛ paanʋ̃ɔ a dãlpʋɔ nyã pɔ tʋ̃ɔ kãan a nɩyɔɔ banyãna?"
40015034	Ka Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Paanʋ̃ɔ aŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tara?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Ayopõi nɩ jɩ̃mɛ bɩ̃lãa."
40015035	Wʋ vɛ̃n ka a nɩbɛ jɩ̃nɛ tẽe.
40015036	Ka wʋ pãa de a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ ayopõi nɩ a jɩ̃bɩ̃lãa ala na wʋ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, tɩ na wʋ ŋma de kʋ a wʋ poturbo, ka ba de põ a nɩbɛ.
40015037	Ba jaa din tɩɩ, ka a poturbo wob a bʋ̃ŋmaar 'yɔ̃ɔ pɛr ayopõi.
40015038	A bala na di ɩn dɔɔr tur anaar, ka pɔbɔ nɩ bibiir nũu ba pʋɔ ɛ.
40015039	Wʋn wa vɛ̃ ka a nɩbɛ yaar baar wʋ kpɛ̃n a gboro na wʋ chen Magadan paal pɔ.
40016001	A Faraseemɩne nɩ a Saduseemɩne wan ɩka ba bɛɛr Yesu kaa na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Wiil sɩ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ na ɩ jɩ̃nɛ na yi a saaju."
40016002	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ala wa ɩ jãanʋɔr lɛ, yɩ ma 'yɛr ɩka a wɛr chaar naa bojũu a saaju mʋ̃ɔ naa.
40016003	Ala wa ɩ bibio lɛ, yɩ ma 'yɛr ɩka saa na wan a dɩna, a julõjuur sɔb naa ka saa koro. Yɩ ma kãan a saaju tɩ 'yɛr ɩka saa na wan bɩɩ wʋ kʋ̃ wa ɛ, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a tẽe nɩ a saaju 'yɛr ma 'yɛr, ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ a dɩna ɛ?
40016004	Yɩn yelbe-ɩrbɛ nɩ sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n tʋ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ka yɩ kaa, yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ka a Jona nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba lɛ ɛ." Be lɛ wʋ bar ba tɩ chen.
40016005	A poturbo ĩin ba tʋ̃ɔ de paanʋ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ na ba gɔ̃ɔ a man gɔ̃ɔn.
40016006	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Saduseemɩne dãbɩl pɔ."
40016007	Ba piel mana kʋrɔ taa, "Sɩn ba waan paanʋ̃ɔ jaa lɛ so."
40016008	Yesu na wa bɔ̃ɔn wʋ 'yɛr naa, "Yɩn sɔɔfʋ na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ 'yɛrɛ ɩka yaa tara paanʋ̃ɔ ɛ?
40016009	Yaa nyɛ bɔ̃ɔ a par sɛrɛ bɩɩ? Yaa tɩɛrtɔ a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu a nɩbɛ tur anũu na di faa tɩ yɩ wob a bʋ̃ŋmaar 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɛr pie nɩ ayi bɩɩ? Yaa tɩɛrtɔ a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu a nɩbɛ tur anũu na di faa tɩ yɩ wob a bʋ̃ŋmaar 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɛr pie nɩ ayi bɩɩ?
40016010	Bɩɩ a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ ayopõi a nɩbɛ tur anaar na di faa tɩ yɩ wob 'yɔ̃ɔ pɛr ayopõi bɩɩ?
40016011	Bo lɛ so ka yaa tɩɛr bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a ba ɩ paanʋ̃ɔ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ ɛ? Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Saduseemɩne dãbɩl yele pɔ."
40016012	Be lɛ ba pãa tɩɛr bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a ba ɩ a paanʋ̃ɔ dãbɩl lɛ ɛ tɩchɛ ba bɔ̃ɔn a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Saduseemɩne wiilfʋ.
40016013	A Yesu na wa kpɛ a Sisariya Filipai paal pɔ, wʋ sʋʋr a wʋ poturbo, "An lɛ a nɩbɛ 'yɛr ɩka a maa Nɩsaal Bie ɩ naa?"
40016014	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Bamɩne 'yɛr ɩka Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suoro, ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr ɩka Elaija lɛ, ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr ɩka Jeremiya bɩɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ."
40016015	Tɩchɛ a wʋ sʋʋr ba, "An lɛ yɩn 'yɛr ɩka n ɩ naa?"
40016016	Ka Simon Pita 'yɛr, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nɩ-iraa, a Nãaŋmɩn Vʋr Bie."
40016017	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Fʋ ju nʋ̃mɔ̃ na Simon, Jona bie! A ba ɩ nɩsaal nɩ nɩrɛ lɛ ir wiil fʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a n Sãa na be a saaju lɛ.
40016018	Maa lɛ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, a fʋ̃ʋ Pita, a par lɛ kʋsɩr pie, a fʋ 'yɛr nyãna pɔ lɛ, ɩn tu bʋɔl nɩbɛ a ba wa sɔɔ de ma ka a kpĩi tẽe kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ba ɛ.
40016019	Ɩn kʋ fʋn a saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ pãn bie, bon 'lɔ jaa fʋn lũ ka a wɛr pɔ, a mɩn lũn a be a saaju, bon 'lɔ jaa fʋn for bar ka a wɛr pɔ, a mɩn for bar a be a saaju."
40016020	Ka wʋ pãa kpãkpãan a wʋ poturbo ɩka ba taa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa ɛ.
40016021	An piel a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a Yesu piel 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ ba ɩka wʋn chen Jerusalɛm tɩ di dɔɔyɛ a nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe nuur pɔ, ka ba kʋ wʋ, ka a ber ata daar a wʋ lɛ ir ɩ vʋr.
40016022	Ka Pita tɔɔ wʋ yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ na wʋ tɩ piel 'yɛrɛ, "N Soro, Nãaŋmɩn kʋ sɔɔ ka a yele nyã ɩ fʋ ɛ."
40016023	Tɩchɛ a Yesu lɩɛb 'yɛr kʋ a Pita, "Tɔɔ lan ka tɩ chɛ ma. Fʋ ɩn Satan, na fʋ ɩ gbɛr ŋme bon kʋ ma. Faa tara Nãaŋmɩn bonsɩ tɩɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩsaal bonsɩ tɩɛr lɛ fʋ tara."
40016024	Ka a Yesu pãa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa bʋɔrɔ na ɩka wʋ ɩ a n poturo, wʋ 'laar a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩ 'mɔɔ a wʋ daa tuo turo nɩ ma.
40016025	A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ faa a wʋ nyɛvʋr na bɔr wʋ naa, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na bɔr a wʋ nyɛvʋr a maa jũu, na nyɛ wʋ naa.
40016026	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ tara naa a wɛr ju bonsɩ a jaa, tɩ bɔr a wʋ nyɛvʋr, bo tʋ̃nɔ̃ lɛ wʋn nyɛ? Bɩɩ bo lɛ wʋn de tɛɛn a wʋ nyɛvʋr?
40016027	A maa Nɩsaal Bie na waan naa Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr nɩ a wʋ malakasɩ wa yab nɩrɛ jaa bon 'lɔ wʋn maal.
40016028	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a yɩ bamɩne na ara a ka kʋ̃ kpi ɛ, tɩ na yɩ nyɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na waara a n nãa difʋ jie."
40017001	A ber ayʋɔb daar, Yesu tara na Pita nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ a wʋ yɛbɛ Jɔɔn don tɔ̃wõo ju a ba tɛɛ.
40017002	Wʋ chil wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a ba niem, ka a wʋ nie nyɩlɛ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ kaar, ka a fuu pɛl nyɩlɛ bũu kaar.
40017003	Mosesɩ nɩ Elaija mɩ wa dũun yɩ ara a wʋ sɛ̃, ka ba wa 'mataa 'yɛrɛ.
40017004	Pita 'yɛr kʋ Yesu, "N Soro, a vɩla na ka sɩn kpɩɛrɛ a ka. Ala ɩ fʋ sɔɔ naa, ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔn sɛɛr ata a ka na, ka fʋ so a ɩ̃sʋɔ, ka Mosesɩ mɩ so a ɩ̃sʋɔ, ka Elaija mɩ so a ɩ̃sʋɔ."
40017005	Wʋn chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ ka a julõjupɩla wa pɔɔ ba naa, ka Nãaŋmɩn kɔkɔr 'yɛr be a julõjuur pɔ, "Nyã lɛ a n Binʋ̃nãa, a n pʋɔ pɛl wʋ naa, yɩ chɛlɛ a wʋ 'yɛr."
40017006	A poturbo na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃ dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba naa ka ba lo kpa tẽe.
40017007	Tɩchɛ ka Yesu wa sɩɩr ba tɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩ ir, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ."
40017008	Ban wa dʋɔ kaa, baa nyɛ nɩrɛ jaa ka a Yesu tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
40017009	Ban wa yi a tɔ̃ɔ ju suro, Yesu kpãa ba naa, "Yɩ taa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa a bon 'lɔ yɩn nyɛ ɛ, tɩ tãn a daar 'lɔ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na lɩɛb ir a kũu pɔ."
40017010	Ka a wʋ poturbo sʋʋr wʋ, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a ɩ ka a nɛɛ wiwiilbe 'yɛr ɩka Elaija lɛ na de nie wa?"
40017011	Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, ɩka Elaija wa naa wa chɔɔr a bonsɩ a jaa.
40017012	Tɩchɛ yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka Elaija den nie wa ka baa bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ ba ɩ wʋn a lɛ na pɛl a ba pʋɔ. Lɛ mɩ lɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie mɩ na di a dɔɔyɛ a ba nuur pɔ."
40017013	Be lɛ a poturbo pãa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suoro 'yɛr lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ.
40017014	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo na wa chen a nɩyɔɔ sɛ̃, daba wa gbur dumo a wʋ niem,
40017015	tɩ 'yɛr, "N Soro, kaa a n bie nɩbaal, kpũgul lɛ wʋ loro na wʋ dire dɔɔyɛ yɔɔ, sɔ̃ɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ wʋ ma lon bũu pɔ bɩɩ kʋ̃ɔ pɔ.
40017016	N tara wʋn waan a fʋ poturbo sɛ̃, tɩchɛ baa tʋ̃ɔ sãa wʋ ɛ."
40017017	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ babãma dẽme, a yɩ sɔɔfʋ na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ, n be a yɩ sɛ̃ naa tɩ tãn dabor? N tara nɩ yɩ kãnyir jɩ̃ ŋmɩnɛ?" Tɩ 'yɛr a daba, "Tɔɔ a bie wa kʋ ma."
40017018	Yesu tãn a sɩdɛɛr ka wʋ yi a bie pɔ, a dẽdẽe daa ka a bie sa.
40017019	A poturbo wan a Yesu tɛɛ sɛ̃ wa sʋʋr, "Ŋmɩnɛ a ɩ ka sɩn ba tʋ̃ɔ dii a sɩdɛɛr bar ɛ?"
40017020	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Bojũu a yɩ sɔɔfʋ ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ. Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩn tara sɔɔfʋ kʋ jɩ̃ a kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ bir, yɩn 'yɛr kʋ a tɔ̃ɔ nyãna, ir a ka chen a be; wʋn ir chen. Tɩ yele jaa kʋ ɩ kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ yɩ ɛ."
40017022	Ban wa lɔ̃ɔ taa a Galilee, Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ban gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a maa Nɩsaal Bie ka n di dɔɔyɛ a nɩbɛ nuur pɔ.
40017023	Ban kʋ maa naa, ka a ber ata daar ka n lɩɛb ir ɩ vʋr." Ban wõ a nɩtɔ̃, ba pʋʋr sɔ̃ɔ naa.
40017024	A Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo na wa ta a Kapenahum, a puorfʋ yir lõpodierbe wa 'yɛr a Pita, "A yɩ wiwile maa yab a puorfʋ yir lõpoo bɩɩ?"
40017025	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, wʋ ma yab naa." Pita na wa ta a yir, Yesu lɛ de nie sʋʋr Simon, "Bo lɛ fʋ tɩɛr?" Ba boo lɛ ma yab a lõpoo kʋ a wɛr ju nãmɩne? A ba bibiir lɛ bɩɩ nɩyor lɛ ma yab?
40017026	Pita na 'yɛr ɩka nɩyor sɛ̃, lɛ Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A lɛ a bibiir son ba mɩ̃ɛ.
40017027	Tɩchɛ saa bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ sɔ̃ɔ a nɩbɛ banyãna pʋɔ ɛ, yɩ chen a man pɔ tɩ lɔb a jɩ̃pɩ̃ɩ, yin wa ir a jɩ̃dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ yɩ yuo a nɛɛ, yɩn nyɛn libir, yɩ de ya a sɩ lõpoo. De a jɩ̃m 'lɔ fʋn dɔ̃ɔ nie nyɔɔ, fʋ̃ʋ wa haa a wʋ nɛɛ fʋn nyɛn libibir, de a 'lɔ yab a sɩ lõpoo."
40018001	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a poturbo wa a Yesu sɛ̃ na ba wa sʋʋr, "An lɛ ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar ba jaa a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ?"
40018002	Wʋ bʋɔl bibile na wʋ vɛ̃ a wʋ ara a ba pɔ,
40018003	tɩ wʋ 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩn baa lɩɛb na yɩ kaara fɩka bibiir kaar ɛ, yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ.
40018004	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɩɩr wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a bibile nyãna kaar, lɛ ɩ a kpɛ̃ɛ gar ba jaa a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
40018005	"Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na de a bibile nyãna a n jũu, maa lɛ wʋ de.
40018006	Tɩchɛ, ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mɩ vɛ̃ naa a bʋ̃bile nyãna na sɔɔ ma ɩ yelbier, a nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, bala 'mɔɔ nɩɛr lũ yɔɔl a wʋ nyĩe pɔ daa 'yɔ̃ɔ a man pɔ, ala sa.
40018007	"Nɛbier lɛ kʋ a wɛr, a bɛɛr kaa na vɛ̃ ka ba ɩ yelbier. Bɛɛr kaa na wa naa, tɩchɛ nɛbier lɛ kʋ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ an tu wa!
40018008	Ala ɩ a fʋ nũu bɩɩ gbɛr vɛ̃ naa ka fʋ ɩ yelbier, ŋmaa wʋ lɔb bar. Fʋn tɩ kpɛ a nyɛvʋr pɔ nɩ nũŋmaa bɩɩ gbɛŋmaa sãn fʋn tara a nuur nɩ a gbɛɛ a jaa ayi tɩ na fʋ tɩ kpɛ a wõm jie a be a bũu na ba kpĩine ɛ.
40018009	Ala ɩ a fʋ nɩbir mɩ vɛ̃ naa ka fʋ ɩ yelbier, 'loo lɔb bar. Fʋn tɩ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ nɩ nɩbifɩɛ sa naa fʋn tara a nɩbie ayi tɩ na fʋ tɩ kpɛ wõm jie.
40018010	"Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn sʋ̃ na yɩ taa kaara a bʋ̃bil banyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔrɔ ɛ, yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ a ba malakasɩ ben a saaju ma kaara a n Sãa niem.
40018012	"Bo lɛ yɩ tɩɛr? Ala ɩ a nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ tara na piir kɔbaa, ka bʋ̃'yen wa bɔr, a ba ɩ wʋn bar a kɔbaa forbir ala a pɛchiin baa pɔ, tɩ yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ a bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa wʋn na tɩ nyɛ wʋ bɩɩ?
40018013	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, 'lɔ wa nyɛ wʋ, nʋ̃ɔ ma kpɛ wʋ naa gar a kɔbaa forbir ala na ba bɔr ɛ.
40018014	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ ɩka a ba ɩ a yɩ Sãa saaju bɔfʋ ɩka a bʋ̃bil banyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ wʋ bɔr ɛ.
40018015	"Ala ɩ a fʋ yɛbɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩ fʋn yelbier, chen tɩ wiil wʋ a wʋ sɔ̃ɔnaa fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a 'lɔ tɛɛ. 'Lɔ wa sɔɔ a wʋ bɔrfʋ, yɩ lɛ ɩn yɛɛr go.
40018016	Tɩchɛ 'lɔ ba wa sɔɔ a fʋ 'yɛr ɛ, tara nɩbʋ̃'yen bɩɩ nɩbɛ ayi chiin, ka a nɩbɛ ayi bɩɩ nɩbɛ ata di a 'yɛr dãasɩɛ.
40018017	'Lɔ wa tɔr a nɩbɛ bala niem, 'yɛr kʋ a pupuorbiir, ka 'lɔ wa chɛnɛ tɔr na waa tu a ba nɛɛ ɛ, fʋ maal wʋ fɩka a lɛ fʋn na maal a nɩyuo, bɩɩ a lõpodier kaar.
40018018	"Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, bon 'lɔ jaa yɩn lũ ka a wɛr pɔ, mɩ lũn a saaju bon 'lɔ yɩn lor bar a wɛr pɔ a mɩ lor bar a saaju.
40018019	"Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a yɩ nɩbɛ ayi tara sɔɔfʋ sʋɔr bon jaa, a n Sãa na be a saaju na kʋ yɩ naa.
40018020	Jie 'lɔ nɩbɛ ayi bɩɩ ata na ara nɩ a maa yuor, n ben a ba pɔ."
40018021	Pita wan wa sʋʋr wʋ, "N Soro, ala ɩ a n tɔ sʋɔ ɩ man yelbier gbɛɛ aŋmɩnɛ lɛ ɩn vɛ̃ bar wʋ? Gbɛɛ ayopõi (7) bɩɩ?"
40018022	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ fʋ a ba ɩ gbɛɛ ayopõi ɛ, tɩchɛ gbɛɛ lɩjaata nɩ pie nɩ ayopõi gbɛɛ ayopõi (77)."
40018023	"A lɛ jũu a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ na nyɛntaa fɩka nãa na bʋɔr ɩka 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ba guor a ba libie kaa.
40018024	Wʋn wa tɩ piel guoro a libie yele ba nyɔɔn ɩ̃sʋɔ na di wʋ turo pie sãn waan a wʋ sɛ̃,
40018025	wʋn kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ yab a sãn ɛ, a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr ɩka ba da 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ pɔɔ nɩ a bibiir nɩ a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa yab a sãn.
40018026	"Ka a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ lo gbur dumo a wʋ niem lɔɔrɔ nuur 'yɛrɛ, 'Tara nɩ ma kãnyir, ɩn yab a fʋ sãma a jaa.'
40018027	A nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kãan a wʋ nɩbaal tɩ vɛ̃ a wʋ sãma kʋ wʋ, tɩ bar wʋ.
40018028	"Tɩchɛ, a daba nyã nɩ wʋ ju na wa yɩ a yõo nyɛ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ sʋɔ na di wʋ toofar kɔbaa sãn, wʋ chɩm a daba kɔkɔr pɔ tɩ 'yɛr, 'Yab ma a sãn fʋn di.'
40018029	"Ka a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nyã mɩ lo gbur dumo tɩ sʋɔrɔ, 'Tara nɩ ma kãnyir, tɩ ɩn yab fʋn a sãn.'
40018030	"Ka wʋ tɔr, tɩ nyɔɔ wʋ chiin tɩ pɔɔ tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn yab a sãn.
40018031	A wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃taaba na wa nyɛ a lɛ wʋn ɩ, ba pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa, ka ba chen tɩ man a jaa kʋ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a lɛ jaa na ɩ.
40018032	Ka a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ bʋɔl wʋ wa sʋʋr wʋ, 'Fʋ̃ʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃putuo sʋɔ. Fʋn sʋɔr ma jũu lɛ so ka n vɛ̃ a sãn bar fʋ.
40018033	Fʋ mɩ kʋ̃ naa kaa a fʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ sʋɔ nyã nɩbaal nɩtãa a lɛ ɩn kaa a fʋ nɩbaal ɛ?'
40018034	A wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ suur ir naa ka wʋ de wʋ tɩr ɩka ba tɩ pɔɔ wʋ ge wʋ tɩ tãn a daar 'lɔ wʋn yab a sãn a jaa.
40018035	"Lɛ mɩ lɛ a n Sãa na be a saaju na ɩ yɩ mɩ, yɩn baa vɛ̃ a yɩ yɛbɛ yelbier bar ɛ."
40019001	Yesu na wa 'yɛr a anyã baar, wʋ yin a Galilee chen Judiya paal pɔ, a Jordan man gɔ̃ɔn.
40019002	Nɩyɔɔ turo wʋ naa, ka wʋ sãa a ba baalsɩ a be.
40019003	Faraseemɩne bamɩne wan a wʋ sɛ̃ ɩka ba wa bɛɛr wʋ kaa, na ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Sɔr ben be ɩka daba wʋ bar a wʋ pɔɔ yele kɔ̃ɔ jũu bɩɩ?"
40019004	Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "Yaa kar a be a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na maal ba a pielfʋ daar 'Maal daba nɩ pɔɔ' ",
40019005	na wʋ 'yɛr, "A lɛ jũu, daba na bar a wʋ sãa nɩ a wʋ ma, tɩchɛ ka 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ pɔɔ ɩ bʋ̃'yen, ka ba jaa ayi ɩ ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen?
40019006	Baa lɛ chɛnɛ ɩ ayi ɛ, tɩchɛ ba ɩn ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen. A lɛ jũu, bon 'lɔ Nãaŋmɩn na 'mataa, nɩrɛ wʋ ta oor aa ɛ."
40019007	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Ŋmɩnɛ ka a Mosesɩ 'yɛr ɩka sɩ kʋ wʋ pɔɔ bar gãn, tɩ bar wʋ?"
40019008	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Bojũu a yɩ nyãkpɩ̃ɛn jũu lɛ so ka a Mosesɩ bar a sɔr ɩka, yɩ bar a yɩ pɔbɔ, tɩchɛ a pielfʋ daar a ba dɔ̃ɔ be a lɛ ɛ.
40019009	A lɛ jũu, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na bar a wʋ pɔɔ, ka ala ba ɩ sɛ̃fʋ jũu tɩ kul pɔɔ yuo, wʋ sɔ̃ɔn a kul taa."
40019010	A wʋ poturbo 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, ala ɩ lɛ lɛ a be a daba nɩ a wʋ pɔɔ, a ba sɛɛ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ kul pɔɔ ɛ.
40019011	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɔɔ a wiilfʋ nyã ka a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ a ba bɔ̃ɔ a par tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
40019012	Bamɩne ben be na ba dɔɔr ɛ, an ɩ lɛ lɛ ba dɔɔ ba ka be, ka bamɩne mɩ a ba taaba lɛ maal ba ka baa dɔɔr ɛ, ka bamɩne mɩ tɔr a kul taa a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ jũu, 'lɔ jaa nɩ na tʋ̃ɔ sɔɔ a wiilfʋ nyã, wʋ sɔɔ."
40019013	Nɩbɛ waan na bibiir ɩka wʋ dɔɔl ba a wʋ nũu na wʋ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ba. Tɩchɛ a poturbo mɩɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na waan ba.
40019014	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩ bar a bibiir sɔr ka ba wa a n sɛ̃, yɩ ta pii ba sɔr ɛ, a banyã taaba lɛ so a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ."
40019015	Wʋ dɔɔl ban a wʋ nuur sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ba, tɩ chen.
40019016	Be lɛ ka nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ wa a wʋ sɛ̃ wa sʋʋr, "Wiwile, bo yelvɩla lɛ ɩn ɩ naa nyɛ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ?"
40019017	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr, "Ŋmɩnɛ a fʋ sʋrɔ ma bon 'lɔ na ɩ vɩla? Nɩbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ ɩ nɩbie. Ala ɩ fʋ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka fʋ nyɛ nyɛvʋr turo a nɛbinsɩ."
40019018	Ka daba sʋʋr wʋ, "A boo?" Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "Ta kʋ nɩrɛ ɛ, ta sɛ̃ ɛ, ta ju ɛ, ta di jir dãasɩɛ ɛ,
40019019	'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ sãa nɩ a fʋ ma, na fʋ mɩ lɛ nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kaar."
40019020	Ka a daba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N tu naa anyãna a jaa, bo lɛ chɛ ma?"
40019021	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ala ɩ fʋ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka fʋ ɩ chɛchɛ, tɩ de a fʋ bʋ̃tarsɩ a jaa da, na fʋ de a libie kʋ a nɔ̃n dẽme, fʋn nyɛn a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ tɩ na fʋ wa turo ma."
40019022	A daba na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃, wʋ chiin naa pʋsɔ̃ɔ bojũu wʋ tara na bʋ̃tarsɩ.
40019023	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ yɩ, an ɩn kpɛ̃ɔ tara sʋɔ na kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
40019024	Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ go, an ɩn kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ ka nyɔɔma na kpɛ kparpĩi bɔɔ pɔ gar tara sʋɔ na kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
40019025	A poturbo na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃, nɛɛ 'maa ba naa ka ba sʋrɔ, "An lɛ na pãa nyɛ faafʋ?"
40019026	Ka Yesu kaa ba tɩ 'yɛr, "Ala na ɩ tuo nɩrɛ sɛ̃, Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ yele jaa ba ɩ tuo ɛ."
40019027	A Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Nyɛ sɩn bar bonsɩ a jaa tɩ wa turo fʋ? Bo sãyar lɛ sɩn nyɛ?"
40019028	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a bonsɩ a jaa bʋ̃paalaa lɩɛbfʋ daar, a maa Nɩsaal Bie na jɩ̃nɛ naa a tɩɩr nãalʋ̃ʋ dakɔɔ ju. Ka a yɩn bala mɩ na turo ma mɩ jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ pie nɩ ayi ju, tɔɔrɔ a Isɩral bala pie nɩ ayi 'yɛr.
40019029	Nɩrɛ nyã jaa na bar a wʋ yir bɩɩ yɛɛr bɩɩ yɛpɔbɔ, bɩɩ sãa, bɩɩ ma, bɩɩ bibiir, bɩɩ puo a maa jũu na nyɛn dɔɔltaa gbɛɛ kɔbaa tɩ tara nyɛvʋr na ba tara baar fʋ ɛ.
40019030	Tɩchɛ a nɩyɔɔ na de a nie na wa ben puor, tɩchɛ ka a puor dẽme nɩ wa de a nie.
40020001	"Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nyɛntãan fɩka daba kɔ̃ɔ na dɔ̃ɔ ŋmaa ir bibio jaa pipi yi ɩka wʋ tɩ bɔ nɩbɛ ka ba chen tɩ kɔ wʋ puo pɔ.
40020002	Wʋ sɔɔ naa ɩka wʋn yab ba naa a lɛ ban na de a bɩbir gbul ka wʋ tara ba chiin a wʋ puo pɔ.
40020003	"A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ lɛ wa do bɩ̃lãa wʋ yɩn tɩ nyɛ a nɩbɛ bamɩne na ara a daa pɔ na baa maala bon jaa ɛ.
40020004	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Yɩ mɩ chen a n puo pɔ tɩ ɩn yab yɩn naa a lɛ jaa na sɛɛn.'
40020005	Ka ba sɔɔ chen. Tɩ wʋ lɛ yɩ go a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa vɩrʋ̃ gar ju sãlsɔɔ nɩ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa suro a tɩɩr pɔ na wʋ tɩ bɔ a nɩbɛ bamɩne mɩ.
40020006	A jãanɔ'maar sɔ̃ɔ, wʋ lɛ yin tɩ nyɛ bamɩne mɩ na chɛnɛ jɛ̃ pɔrɔ jaa. Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, 'Bo lɛ so a dɩna yɩn jɩ̃nɛ ba maala bon jaa ɛ?'
40020007	A ba 'yɛr, 'Nɩrɛ jaa ba sʋɔr sɩ kɔb ɛ.' Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Yɩ wa a sɩ chen a n puo pɔ a yɩ tɩ kɔ.'
40020008	"Jãanʋɔr na wa ta, a puo sʋɔ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kaara a wʋ puo, 'Bʋɔl a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ kʋ ba a ba libie, de nie piel a bala na bɩɛr wa tɩ tãn a bala na dɔ̃ɔ nie wa.'
40020009	"A bala na wa bɩɛr wa ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa den a bɩbir gbul libir.
40020010	A dɔ̃ɔ nie dẽme na wa tɩ wa, ba tɩɛr ɩka ban nyɛn gar a lɛ, tɩchɛ a wʋ kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mɩ bɩbir gbul libir.
40020011	Tɩchɛ ban wa de a lɛ baar, ba vʋ̃n nɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a puo sʋɔ,
40020012	na ba gɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a puo sʋɔ 'yɛrɛ, 'A nɩbɛ banyãna wa bɩɛr wa tɩ fʋ yab sɩ jɩ̃taa, nɩ sɩn na ŋmaa ir nɩ ɔɔr wa tʋ̃ lɛ̃ɛɛ ka mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ ŋme sɩ tɩ mʋrʋ̃.'
40020013	"Ka wʋ lɩɛb sʋʋr a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ, 'N badaba, n ba ɩ fʋ dɛɛr ɛ, a ba ɩ yɩn lɛ sɔɔ ɩka yɩn den a bɩbir gbul libir ɛ?
40020014	De a fʋ libir chiine. Maa lɛ nʋ̃ naa kʋ a puor dẽme nɩtãa a lɛ ɩn kʋ yɩ.
40020015	N ba tara sɔr na de a n libie ɩn a lɛ ɩn bʋɔrɔ bɩɩ? Bɩɩ fʋ tara nyuur nɩ a n maal vɩla?'
40020016	"A lɛ jũu, a puor dẽme na wa ben niem ka a nie dẽme mɩ wa be a puor."
40020017	Yesu na wa pãa duoro a Jerusalɛm, wʋ tara na a poturbo pie nɩ ayi yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ na wʋ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba,
40020018	"Nyɛ, sɩ ben duoro a Jerusalɛm ka ban tɩ de a maa Nɩsaal Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe nuur pɔ.
40020019	Ban de man kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka ba la ma, tʋrɔ ma, chɩrɛ nataar 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma, na ba ge ma, tɩ kʋ ma, ka a ber ata daar ka n ir ɩ vʋr go."
40020020	Be lɛ ka Jebedee pɔɔ tara a wʋ bibiir ayi waan a wʋ sɛ̃ wa lo gbur dumo a wʋ niem na wʋ sʋɔrɔ bon kɔ̃ɔ.
40020021	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Bo lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Vɛ̃ ka a n bibiir banyã ayi ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jɩ̃nɛ a fʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ ka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ jɩ̃nɛ a fʋ gʋbaa jie a fʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
40020022	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Faa bɔ̃ɔ a bon 'lɔ fʋn sʋɔrɔ ɛ. Ban tʋ̃ɔ nyũn a dɔɔyɛ ŋmele 'lɔ ɩn na nyũn ɔ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Sɩn tʋ̃ɔ naa."
40020023	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn tʋ̃ɔ nyũn a n ŋmele tɩchɛ maa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr a buor sʋɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ bɩɩ a n gʋbaa jie ɛ, ka a bala a n Sãa na chɔɔr kʋ tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ."
40020024	A poturbo pie bala na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃, ba nyɛn naa a yɛɛr ayi bala suur.
40020025	Ka a Yesu bʋɔl ba waan wa 'yɛr, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn na ɩka a bala na kaara a nɩbɛ bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ lɛ kaara ba bon jaa pɔ, ka a ba nɩbɛrɛ tʋ̃ɔ ba.
40020026	A kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ be a lɛ a yɩ pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ a yɩ kpɛ̃ɛ, wʋ ɩ a yɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃.
40020027	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ a yɩ nɩdiere, wʋ ɩ a yɩ gbãgbaa.
40020028	Nɩtãa lɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na ba wa ɩka ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ ma ɛ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ ɩ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ na wʋ de a n nyɛvʋr faan nɩyɔɔ yelbier bar."
40020029	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo na wa yire a Jeriko nɩyɔɔ turo wʋ naa.
40020030	Ka a jɔ̃n ayi jɩ̃nɛ a sɔr kõkoor. Ban wa wõ ɩka Yesu lɛ tala, ka ba gboolo, "Sɩ Soro, David Bie wooo ɩ, kaa a sɩ nɩbaal."
40020031	Ka a nɩyɔɔ 'yɛr ɩka ba bar gɔ̃mɔ̃ tɩchɛ ka ba chɛnɛ gboolo, "Sɩ Soro, David Bie wooo ɩ, kaa a sɩ nɩbaal."
40020032	Yesu ara na tɩ bʋɔl ba sʋrɔ, "Bo lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maal kʋ yɩ?"
40020033	Ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Sɩ Soro, sɩ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka sɩ nyɛrɛ."
40020034	Nɩbaal kpɛ̃n a Yesu, ka wʋ sɩɩr a ba nɩbie, ka ba nyɛrɛ na ba turo wʋ.
40021001	Ban wa gbʋrɔ a Jerusalɛm nɩ a Betefagɩ a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ ju, Yesu tʋ̃n a wʋ poturbo ayi,
40021002	na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen a tẽbile 'lɔ na be a yɩ niem, yɩn tɩ nyɛn bʋ̃ɔ ban lũ ka a bʋ̃pɔl ara kɔɔ wʋ, yɩ for yaa waan.
40021003	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ wa sʋʋr yɩ naa, 'Ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ foro a bʋ̃ɔ?' Yɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'A Sɩ Soro lɛ bʋɔrɔ yaa.' Wʋn bar sɔr ka yɩ foraa waan fɔɔ jaa."
40021004	A yele anyã ɩ na ka a na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr na wʋ 'yɛrɛ.
40021005	"'Yɛr kʋ a Jerusalɛm nɩbɛ, 'Nyɛ, a yɩ nãa waara na a yɩ sɛ̃. Wʋ siir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ na wʋ do bʋ̃ɔ. Bʋ̃pɔl bile lɛ wʋ do waara nɩ.' "
40021006	A poturbo chen tɩ tʋ̃ a lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr ɩka ba ɩ.
40021007	Ba waan na a bʋ̃ɔ nɩ a bʋ̃pɔl bile na ba de a ba fɔɔr 'yɩɛr dɔɔl, ka wʋ do jɩ̃nɛ a bʋ̃pɔl ju.
40021008	Nɩyɔɔ 'yɩɛr a ba fɔɔr a sɔr pɔ ka bamɩne mɩ 'mɛl vaɩ 'yɩɛr a sɔr pɔ.
40021009	A nɩyɔɔ bala na be a niem nɩ a bala na turo a puor chɩlɛ na 'yɛrɛ, "Yãan yooo, Nãa David Bie! Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃! Yãan yooo, dãnfʋ wʋ ta a saaju Nãaŋmɩn."
40021010	Wʋn wa kpɛ a Jerusalɛm tẽe pɔ, a nɩbɛ ba jaa ɩrɛ na yulõbʋmm, na ba sʋrɔ, "An lɛ a nyã?"
40021011	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na turo wʋ 'yɛr, "Nyã lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ, Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ na be Galilee."
40021012	Yesu kpɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, na wʋ dire a bala na chiin a bonsɩ tɩ daara nɩ a bala na daara baraa, tɩ na wʋ dara a libitɛɛrbɛ tɛɛbʋlsɩ nɩ a bala na daara a papar dakɔɔr lɔɔrɔ.
40021013	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'A n yir na ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jie,' tɩchɛ 'Ka yɩn maal wʋ ka wʋ ɩ nãnyisɩ sɔɔlfʋ jie.' "
40021014	Jɔ̃n nɩ gbɛrsɩ chen a be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ka wʋ sãa ba.
40021015	Tɩchɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe na nyɛ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ wʋn tʋ̃ nɩ a bibiir na ɩrɛ a gɔ̃mɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir pɔ ɩka, "Yãan yooo! Nãa David Bie." Ka a ba pʋʋr sɔ̃ɔ.
