40021016	Ba sʋɔr a Yesu, "Fʋ wõn a lɛ a bibiir banyãna na 'yɛrɛ ɔ?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, yaa dɔ̃ɔ kar ɩka, 'A bibiir nɩ bipɩlɛ nɛgãma pɔ lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ pɛɛfʋ ɛ?' "
40021017	Wʋ bar ba naa tɩ yi chen a Betanɩ tẽe pɔ tɩ gã a be.
40021018	Wʋn wa lɩɛb chen a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ pɔ a bibio, kɔ̃ kpɛ wʋ naa.
40021019	Wʋ nyɛn kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ tɩɛ na ara a sɔr kõkoor, a wʋ chen tɩ ta ka wɔ̃mɔ̃ ba be be ɛ, tɩ wʋ ɩ va nara tɛɛ. Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a tɩɛ, "Fʋ kʋ̃ lɛ wɔ̃ wɔ̃mɔ̃ go ɛ!" Ka a tɩɛ juɔl kpi ajienaa.
40021020	A poturbo na wa nyɛ a tɩɛ na kpi, nɛɛr 'maa ba naa ka ba 'yɛrɛ, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a tɩɛ ɩ juɔl ajienaa a lɛ?"
40021021	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩn tara sɔɔfʋ na yaa baal ɛ, a ba ɩ a lɛ na tʋ̃ kʋ a tɩɛ nyã tɛɛ lɛ yɩn tʋ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩn gba 'yɛr kʋ a tɔ̃ɔ nyãna, 'Ir suu a man pɔ,' tɩ wʋ̃n ir naa.
40021022	Yɩn wa sʋɔr bon jaa tɩ tara sɔɔfʋ, yɩn nyɛ naa."
40021023	Yesu na wa tɩ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ na wʋ wile, ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Juu nɩbɛrɛ wa a wʋ sɛ̃ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn wile wa sʋʋr wʋ, "Bo kpɛ̃ɔ lɛ fʋ de tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyã nɩ an lɛ kʋ fʋ a sɔr ɩka fʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyã?"
40021024	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N mɩ na sʋʋr yɩn sʋʋrfʋ bʋ̃'yen. Yɩn wa tʋ̃ɔ wiil ma a par, n mɩ na wiil yɩ naa a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kʋ ma a kpɛ̃ɔ ka tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyãna.
40021025	A Jɔɔn na dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ wʋ a sɔr bɩɩ nɩbɛ lɛ kʋ wʋ a sɔr? Yɩ 'yɛr n kaa?" Ka ba piel chɩrɛ taa, "Sɩn be 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ tʋ̃ wʋ wʋn sʋʋr sɩ naa ka bo lɛ so ka saa sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ?
40021026	Tɩchɛ sɩn mɩ 'yɛr ɩka nɩrɛ lɛ tʋ̃ wʋ a ba ɩ ɛ, sɩ joro naa a nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ bojũu nɩrɛ jaa sɔɔ naa ɩka a Jɔɔn ɩn Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ."
40021027	Be lɛ a ba 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Saa bɔ̃ɔ ɛ." Ka a Yesu mɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N mɩ kʋ̃ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kʋ ma a kpɛ̃ɔ ka n tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyãna ɛ."
40021028	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tɩɛr? Daba lɛ tara bibiir ayi, na wʋ chen tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a dɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ, 'N Bie chen tɩ tʋ̃ a n puo tʋ̃mɔ̃ a dɩna.'
40021029	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'N kʋ̃ chen ɛ,' tɩchɛ na wʋ ta sɔ̃ɔ lɩɛb a wʋ tɩɛr na wʋ chen.
40021030	A sãa lɛ chen tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a ayi sʋɔ a lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ, ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'N chen naa,' tɩ na wʋ tɔr.
40021031	"A bibiir banyãna ayi, buor sʋɔ lɛ tʋ̃ a wʋ sãa bɔfʋ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "A dɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ lɛ." Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ a lõpodierbe nɩ a pɔɔ baar na dɔ̃ɔ yɩn nie kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
40021032	Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suoro wan wa wile yɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔr ka yaa sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a lõpodierbe nɩ a pɔɔ baar sɔɔn de wʋ, yɩn sɔɔ wa nyɛ gba yaa lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ.
40021033	"Yɩ lɛ chɛlɛ a sʋkpa ɩ̃sʋɔ. Daba lɛ kɔ wʋ puo na wʋ. Wʋ wɔɔn a puo wʋ jaa jilʋ̃, na wʋ tuu bɔɔ ka ban ma pɔr a wɔ̃mɔ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ na ba nɛŋmɛr ir a kʋ̃ɔ. Wʋ mɛn jie ɩ̃sʋɔ na do ka nɩrɛ na ma do jɩ̃nɛ a be kaara a puo. Wʋ den a puo kʋ nɩbɛ ɩka ba kaara tɩ na wʋ yɔ chen paal yuo pɔ.
40021034	A pɔrfʋ sɔ̃ɔ na wa ta, wʋ tʋ̃n a wʋ gbãgbaar ɩka ba chen a nɩbɛ bala sɛ̃ tɩ pɔr a tɩɛ wɔ̃mɔ̃.
40021035	"Tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ bala nyɔɔ a wʋ gbãgbaar ŋme a ɩ̃sʋɔ, na ba kʋ a ɩ̃sʋɔ tɩ na ba lɔb a ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩ kʋsɩbɛ kʋ.
40021036	Be lɛ wʋ lɛ tʋ̃ a gbãgbaar bamɩne ka ba ge ba a lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju.
40021037	A baaraa lɛ wʋ tʋ̃ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ bie a ba sɛ̃ na wʋ 'yɛr, 'Ban 'yɔ̃ɔ naa a n bie.'
40021038	"Tɩchɛ a pokaarba na wa nyɛ a bie, ba 'yɛr kʋ taa, 'Nyã lɛ ɩ a bʋ̃dire, yɩ ɩ a sɩ kʋ wʋ tɩ de a bonsɩ.'
40021039	Be lɛ ba nyɔɔ wʋ kʋ lɔb bar a puo kõkoor.
40021040	"Pʋ̃pãanyã a puo sʋɔ wa wa, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ wʋn ɩ a pokaarba banyãna?"
40021041	Ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wʋn wan wa kʋ a pokaarba banyã ba jaa tɩ de a puo kʋ nɩyor, a bala na ma sɔɔ ka ba põ a puo bonsɩ a ŋmafʋ sɔ̃ɔ."
40021042	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yaa kar a jie nyã a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr ɩka a, 'A kʋsɩr 'lɔ a mɩmɩɛrbɛ na tɔr bar lɛ ɩ a kʋsɩr ju. A sɩ Soro lɛ tʋ̃ a nɩtɔ̃ ka a sɔb sɩ a nɩbie.'
40021043	"A lɛ jũu n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, Nãaŋmɩn na faan a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ yin a yɩ sɛ̃ kʋ a nɩyor bala na sɔɔ wʋ.
40021044	Nɩrɛ nyã na lo a kʋsɩr nyã ju na pʋrpʋr a, tɩchɛ a wʋ mɩ na kʋ nɩrɛ nyã ju wʋn lo dɔɔl."
40021045	A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Faraseemɩne na wa wõ a wʋ sʋkpar anyãna, ba bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka bala lɛ wʋ lɔɔrɔ a sʋkpar gbɛɛrɛ nɩ.
40021046	Ka ba bʋɔrɔ na sɔr ɩka ba nyɔɔ wʋ, tɩ na ba joro a nɩyɔɔ dãbɩ̃ɛ bojũu ba nyɛn ka wʋ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ.
40022001	Yesu lɛ lɔɔrɔ na sʋkpar kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ na wʋ 'yɛrɛ,
40022002	"A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nyɛntãan fɩka nãa kɔ̃ɔ na maal a wʋ bidaba na kulo pɔɔ paalaa bʋ̃diir.
40022003	Wʋ tʋ̃n a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ɩka ba tɩ 'yɛr a bala wʋn bʋɔl a pɔɔ paalaa jie, tɩchɛ a bala wʋn bʋɔl ka ba tɔr.
40022004	"Wʋ lɛ tʋ̃n nɩyor ɩka ba tɩ 'yɛr a bala wʋn bʋɔl, 'Nyɛ, n maal a pɔɔ paalaa bʋ̃diir baar, n kʋn a n nadar nɩ a napɔl ka yele jaa chɔɔr baar, yɩ wa a pɔɔ paalaa jie.'
40022005	"Tɩchɛ ka ba tɔr ka nyã jaa ma chen wʋ chenfʋ jie, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ chen a wʋ puo pɔ, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ chen a wʋ yar jie.
40022006	Tɩchɛ ka a bala na chɛ nyɔɔr a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ge ba tɩ na ba kʋ ba.
40022007	A nãa suur ir naa ka wʋ tʋ̃ a wʋ sojasɩ ɩka ba tɩ kʋ a nɩkʋrbɔ bala tɩ chʋm a ba tẽe.
40022008	"Tɩ na wʋ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ, 'Yele jaa chɔɔr baar, tɩchɛ a bala ɩn bʋɔl ba sɛɛ ɛ.
40022009	Yɩ yi a tẽe pɔ tɩ bʋɔl nɩrɛ jaa yɩn nyɛ ka wʋ wa a pɔɔ paalaa jie.'
40022010	Lɛ lɛ, a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ yin a tẽe pɔ tɩ bʋɔl nɩrɛ jaa ban nyɛ, a nɩmɩn nɩ a nɩdɛbɛ ka a yir wa sɛɛn nɩbɛ wʋ jaa.
40022011	"Tɩchɛ a nãa na wa kpɛ ɩka wʋ kaa a nɩbɛ, wʋ nyɛn daba ɩ̃sʋɔ na ba su a pɔɔbɩɛl fuu ɛ,
40022012	Ka wʋ suur wʋ, 'N badaba, ŋmɩnɛ fʋ ɩrɛ wa kpɛ a ka tɩ ba su a pɔɔ paalaa fuu ɛ?' Ka a daba kpal a nɛɛ.
40022013	"Ka a nãa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ, 'Yɩ lũ a wʋ gbɛɛ naa nuur na yɩ lɔb wʋ bar yõo a libe pɔ, be lɛ nɩbɛ na kõnõ tɩ ɔɔrɔ nyɩmɛ.'
40022014	"Nɩyɔɔ lɛ ba bʋɔl, tɩchɛ bɩ̃lãa lɛ ban chɛl ir."
40022015	Be lɛ ka a Faraseemɩne guor taa na ba wa bɛɛr Yesu kaa na ba na nyɔɔ wʋ a wʋ 'yɛrbie pɔ.
40022016	Be lɛ ba tʋ̃ a ba poturbo nɩ a nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi a Nãa Hɛrɔd sɛ̃, na ba 'yɛr, "Wiwile, sɩ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka fʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, na fʋ wile Nãaŋmɩn sɔr nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, bojũu faa kaara lɛ nɩbɛ na 'yɛrɛ bɩɩ oor ɛ.
40022017	'Yɛr kʋ sɩ a lɛ fʋn tɩɛr. A tara na sɔr ɩka sɩ yab a lõpoo kʋ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa bɩɩ sɩ ta yab ɛ?"
40022018	Tɩchɛ a Yesu na bɔ̃ɔn a ba pʋtɩdɛɛr jũu, ka ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Yɩn nɛɛr ayi dẽme. Bo lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ bɛɛr ma kaa?
40022019	Yɩ wiil ma a libir n kaa." Be lɛ ba de a libikur waan.
40022020	Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "An foto nɩ an yuor lɛ be a libir pɔ?"
40022021	Ka ba 'yɛr, "A Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa lɛ." Lɛ lɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ de a 'lɔ na ɩ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa sofʋ na yɩ kʋ wʋ, na yɩ mɩ de a 'lɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sofʋ mɩ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn."
40022022	Ban wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃, nɛɛ 'maa ba naa ka ba bar wʋ tɩ chen jaa jomm.
40022023	A bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, a Saduseemɩne na 'yɛr ɩka a kũu pɔ irfʋ ba be be ɛ, ba wan a Yesu sɛ̃ wa sʋʋr wʋ,
40022024	"Wiwile, Mosesɩ sɛb ɩka yɛbɛ wa kpi tɩ bar pɔɔ na ba tara bie ɛ, a wʋ yɛbɛ wʋ kul a pɔɔkʋɔr 'lɔ na wʋ dɔɔ bibiir kʋ a wʋ yɛbɛ 'lɔ na kpi.
40022025	Yɛɛr ayopõi lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be a ka a sɩ sɛ̃ ka a ba kpɛ̃ɛ kul pɔɔ na waa dɔɔ bie ɛ, tɩ kpi tɩchɛ a pɔɔkʋɔr bar ka a yɛbɛ de kul.
40022026	Ka a ayi sʋɔ mɩ de a pɔɔkʋɔr kul baa mɩ dɔɔ bie, tɩchɛ ka wʋ mɩ kpi. A lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ ata tɩ tãn a ayopõi sʋɔ.
40022027	Ba jaa na wa kul a pɔɔkʋɔr nyã lʋɔr taa baar a pɔɔkʋɔr nyã mɩ baar kpi.
40022028	Bala wa ir yi a kũu pɔ, a nɩbɛ banyã ayopõi an pɔɔ, lɛ wʋn ɩ, an ɩ ba jaa kul wʋn lʋɔr taa?"
40022029	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yaa nyɛ yɩn bɔr, bojũu yaa bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn gãma nɩ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ ɛ.
40022030	Nɩbɛ wa ir a kũu pɔ, ba kʋ̃ lɛ kul taa ɛ, tɩ ban kaara fɩka malakasɩ na be a saaju.
40022031	Tɩchɛ a kũu pɔ ir fʋ yele, yaa kar a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka,
40022032	n ɩ naa a Abraham Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Isaakɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Jekɔb Nãaŋmɩn ɛ? Wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn vʋr, waa ɩ Nãaŋmɩn kũu ɛ."
40022033	A nɩbɛ na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃ nɛɛr 'maa ba naa nɩ a wʋ wiilfʋ.
40022034	A Faraseemɩne na wa wõ ɩka Yesu 'yɛr tʋ̃ɔ a Saduseemɩne, ba mɩ lɔ̃ɔn taa.
40022035	Ka a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ na ɩ a nɛɛ wiwile sʋʋr 'yɛrbir bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ bɛɛr a Yesu kaa,
40022036	"Wiwile, A Mosesɩ nɛbinsɩ a jaa pɔ, buor lɛ ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ?"
40022037	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, " 'Nʋ̃ a fʋ Soro Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a fʋ nyãa wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ nyɛvʋr wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ tɩɛr wʋ jaa.'
40022038	Nyã lɛ ɩ a kpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a nɛdɔ̃ɔ.
40022039	A ayi sʋɔ mɩ nɩ nyã, 'Nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ a fʋ kaar.'
40022040	A Mosesɩ nɛɛr a jaa nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ wiilfʋ kpãkpãana na a binfʋ nyãna."
40022041	A Faraseemɩne na wa 'mataa, Yesu sʋʋr ba naa.
40022042	"Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tɩɛr a Nɩ-iraa yele? An bie lɛ wʋ ɩ?" Ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "David bie lɛ."
40022043	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ka a nãa David a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ, a wʋ bʋɔl wʋ ɩka, 'N Soro'? Bojũu wʋ 'yɛr naa ɩka,
40022044	'A Soro 'yɛr kʋ a n Soro, "Jɩ̃nɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, ka n wa de a fʋ dɔ̃dẽme ka ba ɩ a fʋ gbɛɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie." '
40022045	Ala ɩ David bʋɔl wʋn wʋ ɩka, 'N Soro,' ŋmɩnɛ wʋn ɩrɛ wa ɩ a wʋ bie?"
40022046	An yɩ a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ chiine, nɩrɛ jaa ba lɛ haa nɛɛ 'yɛr 'yɛr ɛ bɩɩ lɛ 'la sʋʋr sʋʋrfʋ jaa go ɛ.
40023001	Yesu pãa 'yɛr kʋ a nɩyɔɔ bala nɩ a wʋ poturbo,
40023002	"A nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne jɩ̃nɛ na a Mosesɩ dakɔɔ ju.
40023003	A lɛ jũu, yɩ maala a lɛ ban wile tɩ na yɩ turo, tɩ yɩ ta maala a lɛ ban maala ɛ, bojũu ba maa turo a lɛ ban wile ɛ.
40023004	Ba ma lũn tuor tɩɩr tuo nɩbɛ, tɩ maa sɔɔ de a ba nubir sɩɩr ɛ.
40023005	"Yele jaa ban tʋ̃nɔ̃, ba ma bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka nɩbɛ ba nyɛ ba, na ba ma lũ a fɔɔr a ba jur pɔ, tɩ na ba ma su fuusɩ ban ma sɛ bonsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ jaa vɛvɛɛ.
40023006	Bala wa lɔ̃ɔ taa dire, a ji'yɔ̃ɔnsɩ jie lɛ ba ma nʋ̃ ɩka ba jɩ̃nɛ, nɩ a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir a jibɛrɛ jiir.
40023007	Ala tɩ na ba ma bʋɔrɔ ɩka bama puoro ba a dar pɔ, na ba ma bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩbɛ ba bʋɔlɔ ba, Wiwiilbe.
40023008	"Yɩ ta sɔɔ ka ba bʋɔlɔ yɩ, Wiwiilbe ɛ, nɩkpɛ̃ɛ bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ yɩ tara. Yɩ jaa ɩn yɛɛr.
40023009	Yɩ ta bʋɔl nɩrɛ jaa yɩ, sãa a wɛr pɔ ɛ, bojũu yɩ tara na Sãa bʋ̃'yen na be a saaju.
40023010	Bɩɩ yɩ ta bʋɔl nɩrɛ jaa wiwile ɛ, bojũu yɩ tara na Wiwile bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ na ɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
40023011	A 'lɔ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ a yɩ kpɛ̃ɛ wʋ ɩ a yɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃.
40023012	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'mɔɔrɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ire nɩ, Nãaŋmɩn na suun wʋn pĩlem tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na siir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ Nãaŋmɩn na 'mɔɔ wʋn ka wʋ do.
40023013	"Tɩchɛ nɛbier ben a yɩn nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne na ɩ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme sɛ̃. Yɩ pɔɔn a nɩbɛ var bar a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ. Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ ba kpɩɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ na yɩ pɔɔ var a bala na bʋɔrɔ a kpɛfʋ bar.
40023015	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne na ɩ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme sɛ̃. Yɩ ma yɔn jitɛbɛ nɩ a man pɔ na yɩ tɩ 'yɛr lɩɛb nɩrɛ tɩɛr, yɩn wa tʋ̃ɔ wʋ ka wʋ kaara a yɩ kaar, yɩ ma lɩɛb wʋ naa ka wʋn di dɔɔyɛ a bũu dagel pɔ a yɩ kaar.
40023016	"Nɛbier ben a bala na ɩ jɔ̃n tɩ na ba tɔɔrɔ a jɔ̃n, na ba ma 'yɛr ɩka, 'Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na pɔn a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir a ba ɩ tuo ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na pɔn a sɛlma 'lɔ na be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir a lũ wʋ naa.'
40023017	Yɩ ɩn jɔ̃n na yɩ ɩ jɔlɔ. Buor lɛ ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ, a sɛlma bɩɩ a Nãaŋmɩn yir 'lɔ na maal a sɛlma ka wʋ ɩ a chɛchɛ?
40023018	Yɩ mɩ 'yɛr naa, 'Ala ɩ nɩrɛ pɔn na a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie, a ba tuo ɛ, tɩchɛ ala ɩ nɩrɛ pɔn na a Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ 'lɔ na dɔɔl a jie, a lũ wʋ naa.'
40023019	Yɩn jɔ̃n banyã. Buor lɛ ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ, a kʋfʋ bɩɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie na ma vɛ̃ ka wʋ ɩ chɛchɛ?
40023020	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na pɔn a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie, pɔn wʋ naa nɩ bon jaa na dɔɔl a wʋ ju.
40023021	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na pɔn a Nãaŋmɩn yir, pɔn wʋ naa nɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a be.
40023022	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na pɔn a saaju, pɔn naa a Nãaŋmɩn nãkɔɔ nɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na jɩ̃nɛ a be.
40023023	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne na ɩ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme sɛ̃. Yɩ ma ir a bonsɩ pɔ jiir pie pɔ bʋ̃'yen lɔ̃ɔn badʋʋ gba vaar kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, tɩ na yɩ tɔr a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛr ala na tɩrɛ bar na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔr tufʋ, nɩbaal kaafʋ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ tarfʋ. A anyã lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka yɩ turo tɩ na yɩ taa ire amɩne bara ɛ.
40023024	Yɩn jɔ̃tɔɔrbɔ ba nyã. Yɩ ma chuor a jãajubil bar tɩ ma vɔl a nyɔɔma.
40023025	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne na ɩ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme sɛ̃. Yɩ ma pɛɛn a ŋmanyuraa nɩ a ladiraa a yõo tɩchɛ ka a pʋɔ sɛɛn bɔgar nɩ nyuur.
40023026	Yɩn Faraseemɩne na ɩ jɔ̃n. Yɩ ma dɔ̃ɔ pɛɛ a ŋmanyuraa pʋɔ tɩchɛ ka a yõo mɩ pãa pɛɛ a yõo ka a vɩɛlɛ.
40023027	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne na ɩ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme sɛ̃. Yɩ kaara fɩka yar ban pɩ̃ɛ ka a vɩɛlɛ, tɩchɛ ka a pʋɔ pɔ tara nɩbɛ kɔbɔ nɩ dɛɛr jaa bʋrɔ.
40023028	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a yɩn a yõo, yɩ ɩn nɩtor a yɩ taaba sɛ̃, tɩchɛ a yɩ pʋɔm, yɩ tara na nɛɛr ayi nɩ putuyele.
40023029	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne na ɩ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme sɛ̃. Yɩ mɛn a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ yar, tɩ na chɔɔr a bala na tor yar,
40023030	tɩ na yɩ 'yɛr ɩka, 'Sɩn ta be be a sɩ sãakpãmɩne sɔ̃ɔ, sɩ kʋ̃ naa ta pʋɔ ba kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ɛ.'
40023031	A nɩtɔ̃ jũu yɩ din a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ dãasɩɛ ɩka yɩ ɩn a nɩbɛ bala na kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ bibiir.
40023032	Yɩ baar baar a lɛ a yɩ sãakpãmɩne na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ.
40023033	"Yɩn waa bibiir, ŋmɩnɛ yɩn ɩrɛ wa chɩ̃ɛ a bũu dagel kũu.
40023034	A lɛ jũu ɩn tʋ̃n Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ, yɛ̃n dẽme, nɩ a wiwiilbe, ka yɩ kʋ bamɩne yɔɔl a daa ju, yɩn pɔɔn bamɩne na yɩ fɔb ba a yɩ lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir, tɩ na yɩ pãa tulo yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ ba a tẽn a jaa.
40023035	Ka a na di yɩ a nɩbɛ bala na ɩ a nɩtor ba bɔ̃ɔ yele jaa yɩn kʋ, piel a Abel jɩ̃ɩ sɔ̃ɔ tɩ tãn a Jekariya bidaba Barakiya ban kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie nɩ a puorfʋ jie chara pɔ.
40023036	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ na nyɛn gefʋ a yele anyãna jũu.
40023037	"Pa yɩn Jerusalɛm nɩbɛ, a yɩn na ma kʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na yɩ lɔɔrɔ a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ a yɩ sɛ̃ nɩ kʋsɩbɛ, nyɛ lɛ an ma ɩrɛ ma vɔlaa jɩ̃ ka n ma bʋɔrɔ ɩka n kaal a fʋ bibiir 'mataa fɩka nʋ̃ɔ na ma ũun a wʋ bil, tɩchɛ ka faa bʋɔrɔ ɩka fʋ maal a lɛ ɛ.
40023038	A lɛ jũu n bar a fʋ tẽe kʋ fʋ ka wʋ ɩ dakpolo.
40023039	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩ kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ ma go ɛ, wa tɩ tãn yɩn na 'yɛr ɩka, 'Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃.' "
40024001	Yesu na wa yi a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir pɔ na wʋ chiine, a wʋ poturbo turo wile ɩka wʋ nyɛ lɛ ban mɛ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ka wʋ kaara.
40024002	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Mɩ yɩ mɩ nyɛ naa anyãna a jaa? Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a kʋsɩvɩɛl anyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ lɛ wa chɛnɛ dɔɔl a wʋ tɔ ju ɛ. Ban wa dãn a jaa lɔb."
40024003	Yesu na wa do jɩ̃nɛ a Olive Tɔ̃ɔju, a poturbo wan a wʋ sɛ̃ a ba tɛɛ wa sʋʋr wʋ, "'Yɛr kʋ sɩ a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a anyãna nɩ na ɩ. Bo lɛ na ɩ a jɩ̃nɛ a fʋ waa sɔ̃ɔ nɩ a wɛr baarfʋ daar?"
40024004	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn sʋ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa ta wa bɛl yɩ ɛ.
40024005	Bojũu, nɩyɔɔ na de naa maa yuor waan wa 'yɛrɛ, 'Maa lɛ a Nɩ-iraa,' na ban bɛl nɩyɔɔ.
40024006	Yɩn wa wõn tam, ka ba 'yɛrɛ a tam 'yɛr, yɩ ta mɩrɛ ɛ. A lɛ na ɩ naa, tɩchɛ a wɛr baarfʋ chɛnɛ na be puor.
40024007	Paal dẽdẽme na yin tam, ka a nãmɩne mɩ yɩ tam ka kɔ̃ mɩ lo ka a tẽe jiir amɩne dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
40024008	A dɔɔyɛ anyãna, an kaara fɩka a pɔɔ na ma dɔɔrɔ ka a wõnõ wʋ.
40024009	"Ban pãa nyɔɔr yɩn chiin na ba tɩ pɔb yɩ na ba kʋ yɩ, ka a paalsɩ a jaa 'laar yɩ, yɩn sɔɔ ma jũu.
40024010	Nɩyɔɔ na bar a ba sɔɔfʋ, na ba gar 'yɔ̃ɔ taa na ba 'laar taa.
40024011	Jir ŋmarba 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na wan wa 'yɛrɛ bɛlɛ nɩyɔɔ.
40024012	Nɩyɔɔ nɩ na tɔr Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ, ba kʋ̃ nʋ̃ taa ɛ.
40024013	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ nyã na ara tɩ tãn a baaraa Nãaŋmɩn na faa wʋ naa.
40024014	Ban mʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã a wɛr wʋ jaa ka a ɩ dãasɩɛ a paalsɩ a jaa pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a wɛr pãa baar.
40024015	"Yɩn wa nyɛ naa a yele 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na 'laar na waara nɩ sɔ̃ɔfʋ ka wʋ be a jichɛchɛ 'lɔ nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Danɩɛl na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr. Vɛ̃ ka a nyã na kara bɔ̃ɔ a par.
40024016	Yɩn wa nyɛ a lɛ a nɩbɛ bala na kpɩɛrɛ a Juda, ba jo do a tɔ̃ɔ ju.
40024017	Nɩrɛ jaa na be gar ju, wʋ ta suu a die pɔ tɩ de bon jaa ɛ.
40024018	'Lɔ mɩ na be a puo pɔ wʋ ta kul a yir tɩ de a wʋ fuu ɛ.
40024019	A bɩbir nyãna wa vɩɛ an ɩn tuo kʋ a pɔɔpʋʋr nɩ a bala na tara a bi'yɛnsɩ.
40024020	Yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka a yɩ jofʋ ta ɩ sɩ̃ɛ ɛ, bɩɩ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar ɛ.
40024021	Nãaŋmɩn na maal a wɛr wa tãn a pʋ̃pãanyã, baa di a dɔɔyɛ nyã bʋrɔ ɛ, bɩɩ dɔɔyɛ kʋ̃ lɛ wa jɩ̃ wʋ go ɛ.
40024022	Ala ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn ba ŋmaa a ber ala bar ɛ, nɩrɛ kʋ̃ lɛ chɛnɛ go ɛ. Tɩchɛ a bala wʋn chɛl ir jũu wʋn ŋmaan a ber bar.
40024023	A lɛ daar nɩrɛ wa 'yɛr yɩ ɩka, 'Nyɛ a Nɩ-iraa,' bɩɩ ''Lɔ nɩ nyã,' yɩ ta sɔɔ de ɛ.
40024024	Bojũu jirsɩ Nɩ-irsɩ nɩ jirsɩ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na wa naa wa tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ na ba bɛl nɩbɛ bamɩne ala ɩ ba tʋ̃ɔ naa ban 'mantaa bɛl a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na chɛl ir.
40024025	Yɩ nyɛ, n den nie 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ.
40024026	"A lɛ jũu, bala wa 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka, 'Nyɛ 'lɔ nɩ nyã a dãlpʋɔ ju,' yɩ ta yi a be ɛ. 'Bala wa 'yɛr nyɛ, 'lɔ nɩ nyã a die pɔ,' yɩ ta sɔɔ ɛ.
40024027	A lɛ a saa nyɩɩrfʋ na ma yi a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie na wʋ chaar 'yɔ̃ɔ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ mʋrfʋ jie, lɛ lɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie waa mɩ na kaara.
40024028	Jie 'lɔ jaa bʋ̃kũu na be, be lɛ a sɩdumo ma 'laara.
40024029	"Ajienaa, a ber anyãna a dɔɔyɛ baarfʋ puor, 'A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na lii naa, ka a chuu mɩ kʋ̃ lɛ chaar ɛ, ka a ŋmɛrbie pɔrɔ yire a saaju loro, ka a saaju bonsɩ a jaa dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.'
40024030	"A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ban nyɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na waara a julõjuur pɔ, ka a paalsɩ a jaa na be ka a wɛr pɔ kõnõ. Ka ba nyɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na yi a saaju a julõjuur pɔ, waara nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ tɩɩr.
40024031	Wʋn tʋ̃n a wʋ malakasɩ ka ba pɛɛl a ɩɩl kpɛ̃ɔ jaa na ba bʋɔl a nɩbɛ bala wʋn chɛl ir a wɛr wʋ jaa 'mataa.
40024032	"Yɩ de a pɔlpɔl tɩɛr yele jãn yɛ̃. 'Lɔ wa tʋɔrɔ a vaar, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a tʋl sɔɔ gbʋr naa.
40024033	A lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, yɩn wa nyɛ a yelsɩ anyãna, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a maa Nɩsaal Bie waa gbʋr naa jaa yɛ̃yɛ̃.
40024034	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a pʋ̃pãanyã nɩbɛ kʋ̃ kpi baar ɛ, wa tɩ tãn a yelsɩ anyãna na ɩ.
40024035	A saaju nɩ a wɛr na wa baaraa, tɩchɛ maa 'yɛrbie 'lɔ kʋ̃ wa baar ɛ.
40024036	"Nɩrɛ jaa ba bɔ̃ɔ a bɩbir nyã ɛ, bɩɩ a sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a malakasɩ mɩ gba na be a saaju ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, bɩɩ a Bie ɛ, ka a Sãa tɛɛ ba lɛ bɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
40024037	A lɛ an dɔ̃ɔ kaara a Nowa sɔ̃ɔ, lɛ lɛ an mɩ na kaara a maa Nɩsaal Bie waa sɔ̃ɔ.
40024038	Bojũu sɛrɛ, tɩchɛ ka a kɔ̃paalaa wa nɩbɛ dire na, tɩ nyuro, ka dɔɔr nɩ pɔbɔ kulo taa, tɩ tãn a bɩbir 'lɔ a Nowa na kpɛ a daka bulomtum pɔ.
40024039	Baa bɔ̃ɔn ɛ, tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a kɔ̃paalaa na wa di ba, lɛ mɩ lɛ an kaara a maa Nɩsaal Bie waa daar.
40024040	Nɩbɛ ayi na ben puo pɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn wa de a ɩ̃sʋɔ chiin tɩ bar a ɩ̃sʋɔ.
40024041	Pɔbɔ ayi na 'mantaa nɩɛnɛ jɔ̃ ka a Nãaŋmɩn wa de a ɩ̃sʋɔ chiin tɩ bar a ɩ̃sʋɔ.
40024042	"A lɛ jũu yɩ kaara sʋ̃, bojũu yaa bɔ̃ɔ a bɩbir 'lɔ a yɩ Soro nɩ na wa ɛ.
40024043	Tɩchɛ yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a yele anyã par, a yir sʋɔ ta bɔ̃ɔn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a nãnyie na waara a tɩ̃sɔɔ, wʋ kʋ̃ naa gur ɛ, ka a nãnyie wa kar kpɛ wʋ a yir ɛ.
40024044	A lɛ jũu, yɩ mɩ guro a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, bojũu a maa Nɩsaal Bie na wan a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ yɩn kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔn ɛ.
40024045	"An lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ɩ a yɛ̃ nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ kaara wʋ a yir na wʋ kʋrɔ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ a ba bʋ̃diir a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ?
40024046	An ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nyãna a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wa nyɛ ka wʋ ɩrɛ a lɛ.
40024047	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, wʋn vɛ̃n ka wʋ kaara a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa.
40024048	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nyãna ɩn putusʋɔ na wʋ tɩɛr a wʋ nyãa pɔ ɩka, a n nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kor naa,
40024049	tɩ piel gere a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ bala na be a yir tɩ pãa ma di na wʋ ma pʋɔ a dãnyurbo pɔ,
40024050	a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wa dũu wʋ naa a bɩbir 'lɔ wʋn ba tɩɛr nɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn ba bɔ̃ɔn ɛ.
40024051	Wʋn ŋma wʋn gbʋl gbʋl 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɛɛr ayi dẽme pɔ, be lɛ ban kõnõ tɩ ɔɔrɔ nyɩmɛ.
40025001	"A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ na kaara fɩka pɔɔsarsɩ pie na de a ba fɩ̃tɩnɛ ɩka ba tɩ tuor a pɔɔ paalaa nɩ a wʋ sɩrɛ.
40025002	Ka a ba anũu ɩ jɔlɔ, tɩchɛ ka a ba anũu mɩ ɩ yɛ̃ dẽme.
40025003	A jɔlɔ bala den a ba fɩ̃tɩnɛ tɩchɛ baa de kãa pʋɔ ɛ,
40025004	tɩchɛ ka a ba anũu bala mɩ na ɩ a yɛ̃ dẽme, de kãa pʋɔ a ba fɩ̃tɩnɛ pɔ.
40025005	A pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ na wa kor a waa jũu, gʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ba naa ka ba gã gur.
40025006	"A tɩ̃sɔɔ bɩ̃ɩn lɛ ba ŋme chɛlma tãna 'yɛrɛ, 'A pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ waara, yɩ yi wa tuor wʋ yooo.'
40025007	"A pɔɔsarsɩ pie banyãna vaan ir tɩɛ tɩɛ a ba gonsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba fɩ̃tɩnɛ pɔ.
40025008	A jɔlɔ bala 'yɛr kʋ a yɛ̃ dẽme, 'Yɩ pʋr a yɩ kãa amɩne kʋ sɩ, a sɩ bonsɩ kpĩine naa.'
40025009	"Be lɛ ka a yɛ̃ dẽme bala 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Kai, a kʋ̃ ta sɩ nɩ a yɩn ɛ. Yɩ chen a be ban daara na yɩ tɩ da.'
40025010	"Tɩchɛ, ban lɩɛb chiine a dafʋ jie, a pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ wa naa, ka a bala jaa na chɔɔr 'mataa kpɛ a pɔɔ paalaa kulfʋ jie, tɩ na ba nyɔɔ a pãn pɔɔ.
40025011	"A jɔlɔ anũu bala mɩ wa bɩɛr wa na ba mɩ wa kpooro a pãn 'yɛr, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, yuo a pãn ka sɩ kpɛ.'
40025012	"Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa, n ba bɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɛ.'
40025013	"A lɛ jũu yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ bojũu yaa bɔ̃ɔ a bɩbir bɩɩ a sɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
40025014	"A mɩ lɛ nyɛntãan go fɩka daba kɔ̃ɔ na bʋɔrɔ yɔfʋ na wʋ bʋɔl a wʋ gbãgbaar 'mataa de a wʋ bonsɩ põ ba.
40025015	Wʋ kʋn ɩ̃sʋɔ sɛlbie anũu, na wʋ kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ sɛlbie ayi na wʋ kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ sɛlbir bʋ̃'yen. Wʋ ma kʋn ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa man a wʋ fɔ̃ɔ, tɩ na wʋ yɔ.
40025016	A 'lɔ na de a sɛlbie anũu tɩ yar nyɛ sɛlbie anũu tʋ̃nɔ̃ dɔɔl.
40025017	A 'lɔ mɩ na de a sɛlbie ayi tɩ yar mɩ nyɛ sɛlbie ayi tʋ̃nɔ̃ dɔɔl.
40025018	Tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na de a sɛlbir bʋ̃'yen tɩ tuun bɔɔ de a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sɛlbir ũu.
40025019	"An wa kor bɩ̃lãa ka a gbãgbaar bala nɩkpɛ̃ɛ wa wa ɩka ba guor a sɛlbie yele.
40025020	A 'lɔ na de a sɛlbie anũu waan na sɛlbie anũu wa 'yɛr, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, sɛlbie anũu lɛ fʋ dɔ̃ɔ kʋ ma, nyɛ sɛlbie anũu tɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ n nyɛ dɔɔl.'
40025021	"Ka a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'Fʋ tʋ̃n vɩla, gbãgbamɩ̃ɛ lɛ fʋ ɩ. Fʋ tara na yelmɩ̃ɛ a bʋ̃bile pɔ, ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋn ka fʋ kaara bʋ̃yɔɔ. Wa pʋɔ ma ka sɩ 'mataa dire a nʋ̃ɔ.'
40025022	"A 'lɔ mɩ wʋn kʋ a sɛlbie ayi wa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, 'Fʋ dɔ̃ɔ kʋ ma sɛlbie ayi, nyɛ sɛlbie ayi tʋ̃nɔ̃ lɛ n nyɛ dɔɔl.'
40025023	"Ka a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'Fʋ tʋ̃n vɩla, gbãgbamɩ̃ɛ lɛ fʋ ɩ. Fʋ tara na yelmɩ̃ɛ a bʋ̃bile pɔ, ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋn ka fʋ kaara bʋ̃yɔɔ. Wa pʋɔ ma ka sɩ 'mataa dire a nʋ̃ɔ.'
40025024	"A 'lɔ mɩ wʋn kʋ a sɛlbir bʋ̃'yen wa 'yɛr naa, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, n bɔ̃ɔn na fʋn ɩ nɩbikõo sʋɔ na fʋ ma ŋma a be fʋn ba bʋr ɛ, na fʋ ma wob a be fʋn maa yaar bar ɛ.
40025025	Ala lɛ so ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ma ka de a fʋ sɛlbir tɩ ũu bar. Nyɛ a fʋ sɛlbir.'
40025026	"Ka a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'Fʋ̃ʋ gbãgbaputuo nɩ koro sʋɔ nyã. Fʋn ben bɔ̃ɔn ɩka n ma ŋman a be ɩn maa bʋr ɛ, naa wob a jie 'lɔ ɩn maa yaar bar ɛ,
40025027	a ta sɛɛn ɩka fʋ ta de a n sɛlbir tɩ yɔ̃ɔ a libie yir pɔ, ka maa ta wa lɩɛb wa ka n nyɛ tʋ̃nɔ̃ dɔɔl ɛ?
40025028	" 'Yɩ faa a sɛlbir bʋ̃'yen a wʋ sɛ̃ na yɩ kʋ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara a sɛlbie pie.
40025029	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na tara yɔɔ, ban kʋ wʋn yɔɔ pʋɔ ka ba tara yɔɔ tɩchɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba tara bon jaa ɛ, a bɩ̃lãa 'lɔ wʋn tara gba ban faan yin a wʋ sɛ̃.
40025030	A gbãgbaburbur nyã 'lɔ, yɩ de wʋ lɔb bar yõo be lɛ ban kõnõ tɩ ɔɔrɔ nyɩmɛ.'
40025031	"A maa Nɩsaal Bie wa wa a n tɩɩr pɔ, nɩ a n malakasɩ ba jaa, ɩn wa jɩ̃nɛ naa, a n tɩɩr nãalʋ̃ʋ dakɔɔ ju.
40025032	A paalsɩ a jaa na pãa lɔ̃ɔ taa a n niem, ka n pãa oor a nɩbɛ nɩtãa lɛ pɛchinɛ na ma oor a piir nɩ a bʋʋr.
40025033	Ɩn oon a piir bar a n nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, tɩchɛ ka a bʋʋr mɩ ara a n gʋbaa jie.
40025034	"Ka n pãa 'yɛr kʋ a bala na be a n nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, 'Yɩ wa, yɩn a n Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na sʋ̃ʋ. Yɩ wa kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ, de a yɩ nãbomo wʋn chɔɔr bin gun yɩ a wɛr pielfʋ sɔ̃ɔ.
40025035	Bojũu kɔ̃ dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ ma, ka yɩ kʋ ma ka n di, kɔ̃nyũur dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ ma, ka yɩ kʋ ma kʋ̃ɔ ka n nyũ, n dɔ̃ɔ ɩ sãan ka yɩ ir ma sãan.
40025036	N ba dɔ̃ɔ tara bʋ̃sursɩ ɛ, ka yɩ kʋ ma fuu ka n su, n dɔ̃ɔ bɩɛrɛ ka yɩ sãa ma. N dɔ̃ɔ be pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, ka yɩ wa piir ma kaa.'
40025037	"A nɩmɩn na pãa lɩɛb sʋʋr wʋ, 'Sɩ Soro, nyɩnɛ lɛ sɩ nyɛ fʋ, ka a kɔ̃ kpɛ fʋ, ka sɩ kʋ fʋ bʋ̃diir a fʋ di, bɩɩ ka kɔ̃nyũur kpɛ fʋ, ka sɩ kʋ fʋ kʋ̃ɔ a fʋ nyũ?
40025038	Sɔ̃ɔ buor lɛ sɩ nyɛ fʋ, ka fʋ ɩ sãan ka sɩ ir fʋ a sãan, bɩɩ ka faa tara bʋ̃sursɩ ɛ, ka sɩ kʋ fʋ fuu a fʋ su?
40025039	Sɔ̃ɔ buor lɛ sɩ nyɛ fʋ, ka fʋ bɩɛrɛ, ka sɩ tɩ piir fʋ kaa, bɩɩ sɔ̃ɔ buor lɛ ba nyɔɔ fʋ pɔɔ ka sɩ chen tɩ piir fʋ kaa?'
40025040	"A nãa na 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ maal kʋ a nɩba'yɔ̃ɔnsɩ bala na ɩ a n sofʋ, maa lɛ yɩ maal kʋ.'
40025041	"Tɩchɛ na wʋ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a bala mɩ na be a wʋ gʋbaa jie, 'Pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ turo yɩ naa, yɩ tɔɔ chen be na yɩ tɩ kpɛ a bũu 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na gbɔɔ gun a tɩɩ nɩ a wʋ malakasɩ.
40025042	Bojũu kɔ̃ dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ ma, ka yaa kʋ ma bon jaa ka n di ɛ. Kɔ̃nyũur dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ ma, ka yaa kʋ ma kʋ̃ɔ ka n nyũ ɛ.
40025043	N dɔ̃ɔ ɩ sãan, ka yaa kaa ma sãan kaa fʋ ɛ, n ba tara bon jaa na su ɛ, ka yaa kʋ ma fuu ka su ɛ, ka n bɩɛrɛ, bɩɩ be pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, ka yaa wa piir ma kaa ɛ.'
40025044	"Ka ba pãa mɩ lɩɛb sʋʋr wʋ, 'Sɩ Soro, sɔ̃ɔ buor lɛ sɩ nyɛ fʋ, ka a kɔ̃ kpɛ fʋ, bɩɩ ka a kɔ̃nyũur kpɛ fʋ, bɩɩ ka fʋ ɩ sãan, bɩɩ ka faa tara bon jaa na su ɛ, bɩɩ ka fʋ bɩɛrɛ, bɩɩ ka fʋ be pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, ka saa kaa fʋ ɛ?'
40025045	"Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩn ba maal kʋ a nɩba'yɔ̃ɔnsɩ bala ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ, maa lɛ yaa maal kʋ ɛ.'
40025046	"A nɩbɛ banyãna na chen a dɔɔyɛ 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ jie, tɩchɛ ka a nɩmɩn mɩ chen a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ jie."
40026001	A Yesu na wa 'yɛr a anyãna a jaa baar, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo,
40026002	"Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a chɛn ber ayi ka a Gõl Bar Difʋ na ta, ka ba na de a maa Nɩsaal Bie tɩr ka ba kpa ma a daa ju."
40026003	A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ lɔ̃ɔ taa a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ yir na di Kayafasɩ,
40026004	na ba bʋɔrɔ vuo ban na tu nyɔɔ a Yesu na ba kʋ.
40026005	Tɩchɛ ka ba 'yɛr, a ta ɩ a Gõl Bar Difʋ sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, ka jɛɛr taa ɩrɛ wa ir a chara pɔ ɛ.
40026006	Yesu na wa be a Betanɩ a Simon 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ yir,
40026007	ban wa jɛ̃ dire, pɔɔ kɔ̃ɔ waan na pɩ̃rtɔvɩla nɩ kãnyũu kɔ̃ɔ dafʋ na ba wõnõ ɛ, na wʋ kpaar dɔɔl a Yesu ju.
40026008	A poturbo na wa nyɛ a lɛ, ba nyɛn suur na ba 'yɛr, "Bo lɛ so ka wʋ sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a kãnyũu nyã bar a nɩtɔ̃?
40026009	Fʋn taa den a kãnyũu anyãna da libiyɔɔ de kʋ a nɔ̃n dẽme."
40026010	Yesu na bɔ̃ɔn a ba tɩɛr, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ mii 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ? Wʋ maal vɩla kʋ ma.
40026011	A nɔ̃n dẽme 'lɔ, yɩn nɩ bala ben ka tɩchɛ maa kʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃ sɔ̃ɔ jaa ɛ.
40026012	Wʋn kpaar a kãnyũu anyãna 'yɔ̃ɔ ma, wʋ maal a lɛ chɔɔr ma gun a n ũufʋ.
40026013	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, jie jaa ban wa mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna a wɛr wʋ jaa pɔ, ban 'yɛr naa a lɛ a pɔɔ nyã na ɩ na ba chɛnɛ tara a wʋ tɩɛr."
40026014	A Pie Nɩ Ayi bala ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Judas Isɩkariyot chen a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃
40026015	tɩ sʋʋr ba, "Bo lɛ yɩn kʋ ma ala ɩ n de wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩ nuur pɔ?" Ba sɔr sɛlbie lɩjɛr nɩ pie kʋ wʋ.
40026016	An yɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ wʋ bʋɔrɔ na vuo wʋn na tu de a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba nuur pɔ.
40026017	A bɩbir dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩ naa a Paanʋ̃kõo Lɔ̃ɔfʋ, ka a Yesu poturbo wa sʋʋr wʋ, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ chen tɩ chɔɔr a Gõl Bar nyã Difʋ bar ka sɩ tɩ di?"
40026018	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen a tẽe pɔ, daba kɔ̃ɔ sɛ̃ na yɩ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'A wiwile 'yɛr naa, a n sɔ̃ɔ gbʋr naa, ka maa nɩ a n poturbo na di a Gõl Bar Difʋ a fʋ yir.' "
40026019	A poturbo ɩn a lɛ jaa a Yesu na 'yɛr ɩka ba ɩ. Ka ba maal a Gõl Bar bʋ̃diir.
40026020	A jãanʋɔr na wa ta, Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo Pie nɩ Ayi wa jɛ̃n jil a bʋ̃diir na di.
40026021	Ban wa dire, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ ma."
40026022	Be lɛ ka ba jaa pʋʋr sɔ̃ɔ ka ba sʋrɔ wʋ bʋ̃'yen 'yen, "An ɩn maa lɛ ɔ, n Soro?"
40026023	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "A 'lɔ ɩn 'mataa tun ala bʋ̃'yen pɔ lɛ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ ma.
40026024	A maa Nɩsaal Bie na kpi naa nɩtãa lɛ ban sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ. Tɩchɛ nɛbier ben a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a maa Nɩsaal Bie wʋn din dɔɔyɛ gar nɩrɛ jaa. Bala ta ba dɔɔ wʋ ɛ, ala sa."
40026025	Judas a 'lɔ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ sʋʋr, "An ɩn maa lɛ ɔ, Wiwile?" Ka a Yesu sɔɔ, "Ɔ̃ɔ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ."
40026026	Ban wa dire, Yesu den a paanʋ̃ɔ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan na wʋ ŋma de kʋ a wʋ poturbo, tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ de 'wɔb, a maa ɩ̃gãn lɛ."
40026027	Wʋ lɛ den a ŋmele 'lɔ ban nyuro nɩ, na wʋ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan tɩ lɛ de kʋ ba, "Yɩ jaa yɩ de nyũ.
40026028	A anyãna lɛ ɩ a n jɩ̃ɩ na ɩ a nɛtɩraa ɩn tara nɩ yɩ na tara kpɛ̃ɔ. An kpaar na a faa nɩyɔɔ ka yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ be be.
40026029	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, n kʋ̃ lɛ nyũ a dãa anyãna ɛ, wa tɩ tãn a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩn na 'mataa nyũn yɩ a dãpaalaa a n Sãa nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
40026030	Ban wa yiel a yiel dãn Nãaŋmɩn, ba suun chen a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ ju.
40026031	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ jaa na jon a tɩ̃sɔɔ nyãna tɩ bar ma a n yõ, a maa jũu. A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'Ɩn ŋme naa pɛchinɛ kʋ ka a piir yɛ̃yɛl.'
40026032	Tɩchɛ maa wa ir a kũu pɔ, ɩn dɔ̃ɔ yɩn nie chen a Galilee."
40026033	Ka a Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ala ɩ ba jaa sɔɔn bar fʋ a fʋ jũu, maa 'lɔ kʋ̃ bar fʋ ɛ."
40026034	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a Pita, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, ɩka a tɩ̃sɔɔ nyãna a nɔrdɔ̃ɔ kʋ̃ kõ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka fʋ chiir ma gbɛɛ ata."
40026035	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ɩka, "Ala ɩ maa nɩ fʋ̃ʋ na 'mataa kpi gba, tɩ n kʋ̃ 'yɛr ɩka n ba bɔ̃ɔ fʋ ɛ." Ka a poturbo bala mɩ na chɛ 'yɛr a lɛ nɛ.
40026036	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo chen a jie 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Getɩsemanɩ, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ jɩ̃nɛ a kana tɩchɛ ka n chen tɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn."
40026037	Be lɛ wʋ tara Pita nɩ Jebedee bibiir ayi ka a wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ jaa ka tɩɛr nyɔɔ wʋ.
40026038	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N tɩɛr sɔ̃ɔ naa, tɩ nyɛtãan kũn, yɩ jɩ̃nɛ a ka na gu ma."
40026039	Wʋ chen a niem bɩ̃lãa tɩ lo kpa tẽe sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ, "N Sãa ala ɩ a tara naa ɩfʋ kɔ̃ɔ, vɛ̃ ka a dɔɔyɛ ŋmele nyãna po ma. Tɩchɛ a ta ɩ lɛ maa na bʋɔrɔ ɛ, tɩ a ɩ a lɛ fʋ̃ʋ na bʋɔrɔ."
40026040	Wʋ lɩɛb wa a poturbo sɛ̃ wa nyɛ ka ba guro. Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A mɔ̃ yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ jɛ̃ bɩ̃lãa jaa gu ma ɛ?
40026041	Yɩ jɛɔ chɛlɛ, na yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka a bɛɛr kaa ta wa nyɔɔ yɩ ɛ. A ba tɩɛr bʋɔrɔ naa tɩchɛ ka a ba ɩ̃gãma ba tʋɔr ɛ."
40026042	Wʋ lɛ chen a gbɛɛ ayi sʋɔ tɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn. "N Sãa, ala ɩ a dɔɔyɛ ŋmele nyã kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ po ma ɛ, ka maa ba nyũn wʋ ɛ, fʋ̃ʋ bɔfʋ wʋ ɩ."
40026043	Wʋ lɛ wan wa nyɛ ka ba chɛnɛ guro, bojũu gʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ba naa.
40026044	Be lɛ wʋ lɛ bar ba tɩ chen a gbɛɛ ata sʋɔ tɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn a lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju.
40026045	Wʋ lɩɛb wa a poturbo sɛ̃ wa sʋʋr ba, "Yɩ chɛnɛ na gã guro na yɩ pɛnɛ wɛ? Nyɛ, a sɔ̃ɔ ta naa ka ban gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a maa Nɩsaal Bie de wʋ kʋ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ.
40026046	Yɩ vaa ir ka sɩ chen. Yɩ nyɛ a gagaraa na waara."
40026047	A Yesu na chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ, ka Judas na ɩ a wʋ poturbo Pie nɩ Ayi ɩ̃sʋɔ, tɩ daasãa nɩ nɩbɛ na yi a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃ waara nɩ sɔbɛrɛ nɩ dakʋrsɩ a wʋ sɛ̃.
40026048	A Judas dɔ̃ɔ man ba ɩka, a 'lɔ wʋn tɩ puor tɩ mʋʋr a kɔtɩr 'lɔ lɛ, yɩ nyɔɔ wʋ.
40026049	Ban wa tɩ ta, Judas pɔɔn chen tɩ 'yɛr, "Wiwile, n puor fʋ naa," tɩ mʋʋr a Yesu kɔtɩr.
40026050	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N badaba, tʋ̃ a lɛ fʋn bʋɔrɔ ɩka fʋ tʋ̃." Be lɛ ba wa nyɔɔ a Yesu.
40026051	Be lɛ ka a Yesu poturbo ɩ̃sʋɔ na ara gbʋr wʋ vʋ̃ɔ a sʋɔ chen a Juu dẽme bɔɔrlo nãa gbãgbaa toor ŋmaa.
40026052	Be lɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "De a sʋɔ su a sʋkpa pɔ, bala na jɛɛrɛ nɩ a sʋɔ na kpin a sʋɔ kũu.
40026053	Fʋ tɩɛr ɩka n kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bʋɔl a n Sãa ka wʋ sʋ̃ʋ ma nɩ a malakasɩ gbulo pie nɩ ayi bɩɩ?
40026054	Tɩchɛ ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an ɩrɛ wa ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãma na 'yɛr ɩka a nɩtɔ̃ lɛ na ɩ?"
40026055	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, a Yesu sʋʋr a nɩyɔɔ bala, "A mɔ̃ nɩbier lɛ n ɩ ka yɩ waan sʋʋr nɩ dakʋrsɩ a n nyɔɔ fʋ jie wɛ? Bɩbir jaa lɛ n ma jɩ̃nɛ wile yɩ a puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, tɩ yaa nyɔɔ ma ɛ.
40026056	Tɩchɛ a ɩ naa a lɛ ka a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn gãma pɔ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ." Be lɛ ka a Yesu poturbo ba jaa bar wʋ tɩ jo.
40026057	A bala na nyɔɔ a Yesu, chiin wʋ naa a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãa Kayafasɩ sɛ̃, ka a nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ ba jaa wa lɔ̃ɔ taa.
40026058	Tɩchɛ ka Pita be a puor jaa turo, na wʋ tɩ kpɛ a bɔɔrlo nãa yir bɛchaar pɔ, tɩ lɔ̃ɔ jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a gugurbo, ɩka wʋ nyɛ lɛ an na baar.
40026059	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ nɩbɛrɛ pãa bʋɔrɔ jir ŋmarba ka ba na ŋmaa jire 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, ka ba na tu a be kʋ a Yesu.
40026060	Tɩchɛ baa nyɛ yele jaa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ. Nɩyɔɔ daan yi ŋma jiryɔɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, tɩchɛ ka a ba 'yɛrbie ɩ jirsɩ. A baaraa nɩbɛ ayi daan yi
40026061	na ba 'yɛr ɩka, "A daba nyãna lɛ 'yɛr ɩka, 'Ɩn tʋ̃ɔ ŋmɛr a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir nyãna bar tɩ de ber ata lɛ mɛn wʋ.' "
40026062	A be lɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãa ir ara tɩ sʋʋr a Yesu, "Faa tara 'yɛr jaa na 'yɛr bɩɩ? Bo dãasɩɛ lɛ a anyã ban dire dɔɔlɔ fʋ?"
40026063	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu ɩ jaa gbul. Be lɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãa 'yɛr, "N sʋrɔ fʋ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ a vʋr niem, ɩka fʋ 'yɛr kʋ sɩ, ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie."
40026064	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ɔ̃ɔ, a lɛ nɛ fʋn 'yɛr lɛ. Tɩchɛ yɩ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ ɩka daar kɔ̃ɔ, yɩn nyɛn a maa Nɩsaal Bie na jɩ̃nɛ a Kpɛ̃ɔ Sʋɔ nũsʋ̃ɔ jie. Yɩ mɩ na lɛ nyɛ ma naa ka n yɩ a julõjuur pɔ waara."
40026065	Ka a bɔɔrlo nãa tɔɔ a fuu chɩɛr tɩ 'yɛr, "Wʋ sɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn yuor. Bo lɛ so sɩn chɛnɛ bʋɔrɔ dãasɩdirbe? Yɩ wõn wʋ tʋ Nãaŋmɩn.
40026066	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tɩɛr?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Wʋ sɛɛn kũu."
40026067	Ba chir nataar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ a nie pɔ, tɩ ma gbul nũu ŋmen wʋ, ka bamɩne mɩ ma 'ma wʋ,
40026068	tɩ sʋʋr, "Nɩ-iraa, ala ɩ fʋ bɔ̃ɔn yele jaa wiil sɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ŋme fʋ?"
40026069	Pita jɩ̃nɛ naa a yõo a bɛchaar pɔ. Ka a gbãgbapɔɔbile ɩ̃sʋɔ wa a wʋ sɛ̃ wa 'yɛr, "Fʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ turo a Yesu na yi a Galilee."
40026070	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ chiir a ba jaa niem tɩ 'yɛr, "N ba bɔ̃ɔ a 'yɛr 'lɔ par fʋn 'yɛrɛ ɛ."
40026071	Wʋn wa tɩ ara a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ, a pɔɔbile ɩ̃sʋɔ nyɛ wʋ naa na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ na ara a be, "A daba nyã mɩ dɔ̃ɔ turo a Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ."
40026072	Be lɛ a Pita lɛ chiir pɔ tɩ 'yɛr ɩka, "N ba bɔ̃ɔ a daba nyãna ɛ."
40026073	A ba kor ɛ, ka a bala na ara gbʋr a Pita mɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, fʋ ɩ naa a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ. A fʋ kɔkɔr yin fʋn chãa pɔ."
40026074	Be lɛ ka a Pita pɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩ mɩ pɔrɔ kʋrɔ ba 'yɛrɛ ɩka, "N ba bɔ̃ɔ a daba nyãna ɛ." Ka a nɔraa mɩ tɔ̃ɔ kõ.
40026075	Be lɛ ka Pita tɩɛr tɔ a lɛ a Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, "Fʋn chiir ma naa gbɛɛ ata tɩchɛ ka a nɔraa kõ." Ka a Pita ir yi a yõo tɩ kõ nɩbaal kõn.
40027001	A wɛr na wa chaar bibio, a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa guor lɛ ban na ɩ kʋ a Yesu.
40027002	Ba lũ wʋn tara chiin a paal Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Pilate sɛ̃.
40027003	Judas na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ na wa nyɛ ɩka ba tɔɔr a Yesu 'yɛr guor a wʋ kʋfʋ, wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa ka wʋ lɛ lɩɛb a libibie lɩjɛr nɩ pie na wʋ tɩ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ.
40027004	Tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, "N maal yelbier nɩ ɩn gar 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ na ba maal yelbier jaa ɛ." Tɩchɛ ka ba 'yɛr, "Sɩ baka ba lɛ ɛ? Fʋ 'yɛr a ɩ."
40027005	Wʋ den a libie lɔb bar a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir pɔ, tɩ na wʋ yi tɩ yɔɔl miir.
40027006	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ wob a libie na ba 'yɛr ɩka a ba sɛɛ ɩka sɩ de yaa 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir libie pɔ ɛ, bojũu a ɩn jɩ̃ɩ libie.
40027007	Ban wa guor taa baar, ba den a libie dãn a lamɩɛr wɛr a jie ban ma ũno sãanba.
40027008	Lɛ lɛ so ka nɩbɛ bʋɔlɔ a jie nyã, "Jɩ̃ɩ Wɛr," wa tãn dɩna.
40027009	A ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Jeremiya na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, "Ba den a libibie lɩjɛr nɩ pie a lɛ a Isɩral nɩbɛ na sɔɔ de,
40027010	na ba dãn a lamɩɛr wɛr nɩtãa lɛ a sɩ Soro na 'yɛr."
40027011	Yesu na wa ara a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Pilate niem, wʋ sʋʋr wʋ naa, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa ɔ?" Ka a Yesu 'yɛr "Ɔ̃ɔ, a lɛ nɛ fʋn 'yɛr lɛ."
40027012	A bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wʋ yuor, waa 'yɛr 'yɛr jaa ɛ.
40027013	Be lɛ a Pilate sʋʋr wʋ, faa 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr jaa wɛ? Nyɛ lɛ ban sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ yuor jɩ̃?
40027014	Tɩchɛ a Yesu ba haa nɛɛ sɔɔ wʋ nɩ a ala a jaa ban 'yɛrɛ dɔɔlɔ wʋ ɛ, ka a 'maa a Pilate nɛɛ.
40027015	A lɔ̃ɔ difʋ sɔ̃ɔ wa ta, ba ma 'yɛr ɩka a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Pilate wʋ ir nɩrɛ 'lɔ a nɩbɛ na bʋɔrɔ a pɔɔ fʋ die pɔ bar.
40027016	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, ba pɔɔn daputuo sʋɔ kɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ jaa na bɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ di Barabasɩ.
40027017	A lɛ a nɩyɔɔ na wa lɔ̃ɔ taa, Pilate sʋʋr ba naa, "An lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n yuo kʋ yɩ, Barabasɩ bɩɩ Yesu, a 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Nɩ-iraa?"
40027018	Bojũu wʋ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a nyuur ban tara nɩ a Yesu lɛ so ban nyɔɔ wʋ waan a wʋ sɛ̃.
40027019	A Pilate na wa jɩ̃nɛ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ dakɔɔ ju, a wʋ pɔɔ tʋ̃n 'yɛr wʋ, "Taa ɩrɛ wa ɩrɛ a daba 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na ba maal bon jaa yele jaa ɛ, bojũu jãa, n din dɔɔyɛ jãn pɔ nɩ a wʋ yele."
40027020	Tɩchɛ a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩyɔɔ ɩka ba sʋɔr ka wʋ yuo Barabasɩ bar, tɩ kʋ a Yesu.
40027021	Ka a Nãa Pilate lɛ bɔ̃ɔ sʋʋr ba go, "A nɩbɛ banyã ayi, buor lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n yuo kʋ yɩ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Barabasɩ."
40027022	Ka a Nãa Pilate sʋʋr ba, "Tɩ n ɩ ŋmɩnɛ nɩ a 'lɔ yɩn bʋɔlɔ a Nɩ-iraa?" Ka ba jaa 'yɛr, "Kpa wʋ a daa ju."
40027023	Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Bo yelbier lɛ wʋ ɩ? Bo dɛɛr lɛ wʋ maal?" Tɩchɛ ka ba tãna kpɛ̃ɔ jaa 'yɛrɛ, "Kpa wʋ a daa ju."
40027024	A Pilate na wa nyɛ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ yele jaa ɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ wɩlɛwɩlɛ jaa tɩ gar, ka wʋ de kʋ̃ɔ pɛɛn a wʋ nuur a nɩyɔɔ niem, tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Maa ba pʋɔ a daba nyã kũu pɔ ɛ. Yɩn sɛ̃ lɛ a be."
40027025	Be lɛ ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa 'mataa 'yɛr, "Vɛ̃ ka a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ dɔɔl a sɩn nɩ a sɩ bibiir ju."
40027026	Be lɛ wʋ yuo a Barabasɩ kʋ ba. Wʋ vɛ̃ naa ka ba fɔb a Yesu tɩ wʋ de wʋ kʋ a sojasɩ ka ban tɩ kpa a daa ju.
40027027	Be lɛ ka a sojasɩ tara a Yesu tɩ kpɛ̃n a nãa yir kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ pɔ, tɩ bʋɔl a ba taaba sojasɩ lɔ̃ɔ taa.
40027028	Ba yaar a wʋ bonsɩ bar tɩ de fuu jɩɛ su wʋ,
40027029	na ba lɛ de gʋʋr wob nãa jupil kaar su wʋ. Ba den dãgbal 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ a nũsʋ̃ɔ pɔ, na ba gbur dumo a wʋ niem laara wʋ, "Yãan yooo, Juu nɩbɛ nãa!"
40027030	Ba ma chɩr nataar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ tɩ de daa ŋmen wʋ a ju pɔ.
40027031	Ban wa la wʋ a nɩtɔ̃ wa baar, ba yãan a fuu jie 'lɔ bar tɩ de a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ fuu su wʋ, na ba pãa de wʋ chiin ɩka ba tɩ kpa a daa ju.
40027032	Ban wa yi a sɔr pɔ, ba nyɛn daba na yi Sirenɩ ka a wʋ yuor di Simon, ka ba nyɔɔ wʋ fɩr wʋ ka wʋ tuo a Yesu daa.
40027033	Ba tɩ tãn jie ban bʋɔlɔ Gɔlgɔta, a par lɛ ɩka, Julaa Jie.
40027034	Ba den tɩ̃ɩtuo 'yɔ̃ɔ dãa pɔ ɩka a Yesu wʋ nyũ, tɩ wʋn wa lɛm kaa, wʋ tɔr bar.
40027035	Ban wa kpa wʋ a daa ju baar, ba põ naa a wʋ fɔɔr ŋmen gbãm bɔ̃ɔn ala ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa nɩ na di,
40027036	tɩ na ba jɩ̃nɛ a jie pire wʋ.
40027037	Ba sɛb a yele 'lɔ jũu ban kʋn wʋ mar a daa ju ɩka, NYƐ A YESU, A JUU NƖBƐ NÃA.
40027038	Ba mɩ kpan nɩfarba ayi a dabãbɩ̃nsɩ mɩ ju, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ be a Yesu nũsʋ̃ɔ jie ka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ be a wʋ gubaa jie.
40027039	A bala na tala a be tʋrɔ wʋ, na ba vavire jur
40027040	'yɛrɛ, "A fʋ̃ʋ na 'yɛr ɩka fʋn ŋmɛr a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir tɩ de ber ata mɛn, faa a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ. Ala ɩ fʋ ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, wa suu a daa ju."
40027041	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ mɩ laara wʋ,
40027042	na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Wʋ faan nɩbɛ bamɩne, tɩ wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ faa a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ a Isɩral Nãa, wʋ wa suu a daa ju a pʋ̃pãanyãna, ka sɩ sɔɔ de wʋ.
40027043	Wʋ sɔɔn Nãaŋmɩn. Vɛ̃ ka Nãaŋmɩn faa wʋ a pʋ̃pãanyãna, bojũu wʋ 'yɛr naa ɩka wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn Bie."
40027044	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a nɩfarba ayi bala mɩ ban kpa gbʋr wʋ, mɩ tʋ wʋ.
40027045	A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa ara gar ju sãlsɔɔ, a wɛr wʋ jaa sɔb naa tɩ tãn a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ balfʋ sɔ̃ɔ.
40027046	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a Yesu chɩɩr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa na wʋ 'yɛr, "Ɛloɩ, Ɛloɩ, lama sabakatanɩ." A par lɛ ɩka "N Nãaŋmɩn, n Nãaŋmɩn, bo lɛ so fʋn lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ ma?"
40027047	A nɩbɛ bala na ara gbʋr wʋ, na wa wõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr, ka ba 'yɛr ɩka, "Elaija lɛ wʋ bʋɔlɔ."
40027048	Ajienaa ka a daba ɩ̃sʋɔ jo chen tɩ 'mɔɔ sapɔ 'lɔr a dãmiir amɩne pɔ, na wʋ char daa pɔ, de kʋ a Yesu ɩka wʋ mʋʋr.
40027049	Tɩchɛ ka bamɩne 'yɛr, "Yɩ bar a sɩ kaara, Elaija na wa yɔɔ wʋ naa bɩɩ."
40027050	Be lɛ a Yesu chɩɩr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa tɩ ŋmaa a vʋʋr.
40027051	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir pɔ, ban lũ fɔbaa chɩɛr a saaju tɩ gbem a par. Ka a tẽe dãm, ka a kʋsɩbɛ mɩ ŋmɛr ŋmɛr.
40027052	A yar mɩ yuo yuor, ka a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ bamɩne na dɔ̃ɔ kpi, jɛɔ.
40027053	Ban wa yi a ba yar pɔ a lɛ, ka a Yesu na wa ir a kũu pɔ baar, ka ba pãa kpɛ a tẽchɛchɛ pɔ, ka nɩyɔɔ jaa tɩ nyɛ ba.
40027054	A sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a bala wʋn ara nɩ na ba pire a Yesu, nyɛn a wɛr na dãm nɩ a lɛ jaa na ɩ, ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba, ka ba 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ, a daba nyã ɩn a Nãaŋmɩn Bie."
40027055	Pɔɔ yɔɔ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ be a be ara tɛɛr jaa kaara, bala lɛ dɔ̃ɔ tu wʋ yin a Galilee na ba sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ.
40027056	A pɔbɔ banyãna pɔ lɛ Mɛɛr na yi Magdala, nɩ Mɛɛr na ɩ Jemesɩ nɩ Josefʋ ma, nɩ a Jebedee bibiir ma.
40027057	A jãanʋɔr na wa ta, a taraa sʋɔ kɔ̃ɔ na yɩ Arimatɩya ban bʋɔlɔ Josefʋ, wʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a Yesu poturo.
40027058	Wʋ chen a Pilate sɛ̃ tɩ sʋɔr a Yesu ɩ̃gãn. Ka a Pilate bar sɔr ka ba yɔɔ a Yesu kʋ wʋ.
40027059	A Josefʋ yɔɔn a ɩ̃gãn pil fɔpɩla,
40027060	kul tɩ ũu a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yaa paalaa pɔ wʋn chɩ a kʋsɩr pɔ. Wʋ bil kʋsɩr wa pɔɔ a yaa nɛɛ tɩ na wʋ kul.
40027061	Mɛɛr na yi Magdala nɩ a Mɛɛr ɩ̃sʋɔ ben be jɩ̃nɛ a yaa puor.
40027062	A Chɔɔrfʋ Bɩbir ka a wɛr na chaar ka a ɩ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir lɛ, a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Faraseemɩne chen tɩ 'yɛr a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Pilate,
40027063	"Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, sɩ lɛ tɩɛr a lɛ a jir ŋmara 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr wʋn dɔ̃ɔ chɛnɛ, 'Ɩka ber ata daar ɩn lɛ lɩɛb ir ɩ vʋr.'
40027064	A lɛ jũu vɛ̃ ka ba gu a yaa tɩ tãn a ber ata daar, ka ala ba ɩ lɛ ɛ, a wʋ poturbo na chen tɩ ju a ɩ̃gãn a yaa pɔ, tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ ɩka, 'lɔ lɛ ir a kũu pɔ, ka a bɛlfʋ taa ɩ dɛɛr gar a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɛ."
40027065	Ka a Pilate 'yɛr, "Yɩ de gugurbo ka ba tɩ gu a yaa a lɛ yɩn bɔ̃ɔ."
40027066	Be lɛ ba tara a gugurbo chiin ka ba tɩ bɛ a yaa bɔɔ pɔɔ, tɩ na ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a kʋsɩr jɩ̃nɛ, tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ ka a gugurbo ara gu.
40028001	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir na wa baar, ka a na ɩ a Pɛ̃nfʋ divɩɛ bio daar a wɛr na wa chaara wa la la la, Mɛɛr na yi a Magdala nɩ a Mɛɛr ɩ̃sʋɔ yin chen ɩka ba tɩ kaa a yaa.
40028002	Be lɛ ka a tẽe dãm kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, ka a ɩ Nãaŋmɩn malaka lɛ yi a saaju suu wa bil a kʋsɩr bar a yaa nɛɛ tɩ do jɩ̃nɛ.
40028003	A wʋ nie nyɩlɛ saa nyɩɩrfʋ kaar, ka a wʋ bʋ̃sursɩ pɛl jaa pɩlpɩl.
40028004	Dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ̃n a bala na ara kaara, ka ba gĩem ara kũn kaar.
40028005	A malaka 'yɛr kʋ a pɔbɔ, "Yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, n bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a Yesu 'lɔ ban kpa a daa ju lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ.
40028006	Waa be ka ɛ. Wʋ ir naa ɩ vʋr nɩtãa a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr. Yɩ wa muul kaa a jie wʋn gã.
40028007	Yɩ chen fɔɔ jaa na yɩ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, 'Wʋ lɩɛb ir a kũu pɔ, na wʋ de yɩ nie chiine a Galilee. Be lɛ yɩn tɩ nyɛ wʋ.' N pãa 'yɛr kʋ yɩ."
40028008	A pɔbɔ banyãna yin a yaa par nɩ dãbɩ̃ɛ jo fɔɔ jaa nɩ pʋpɛl chen ɩka ba tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo.
40028009	Be lɛ ka ajienaa, ka a ɩ Yesu lɛ tuor puor ba, ka ba lo kpa a wʋ niem nyɔɔ a wʋ gbɛɛ puor wʋ.
40028010	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, "Yɩ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a n yɛɛr ɩka ba chen a Galilee, be lɛ ban tɩ nyɛ ma."
40028011	A pɔbɔ na wa chiine, a sojasɩ bamɩne na dɔ̃ɔ guro a yaa kpɛ̃n a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ pɔ, tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ a lɛ jaa na ɩ.
40028012	A bɔɔrlo nãa nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛrɛ na wa lɔ̃ɔ taa, ba guor taa de libiyɔɔ kʋ a sojasɩ
40028013	tɩ na ba 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ 'yɛr ɩka, 'A wʋ poturbo lɛ wa ju a wʋ ɩ̃gãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn chɛnɛ gã guro.'
40028014	Ala ɩ a 'yɛr nyã wa lon a Nãa Pilate toor pɔ, sɩn maal wʋ naa ka a wʋ pʋɔ pɛl a sɩ ir yɩ yin wõm pɔ."
40028015	A sojasɩ den a libie tɩ na ba ɩ a lɛ ban 'yɛr ɩka ba ɩ. A Juu nɩbɛ ma chɛnɛ na 'yɛr a yele nyãna a dɩna.
40028016	A poturbo pie nɩ bʋ̃'yen chen a Galilee a tɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ju a Yesu na wiil ba ɩka ba do.
40028017	Ban wa nyɛ wʋ, ba gbur dumo na ba puor wʋ tɩchɛ ka bamɩne chɛnɛ baala.
40028018	Ka a Yesu wa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A n Sãa den a kpɩ̃ɛn ala a jaa na be a saaju, nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn ala a jaa na be a wɛr pɔ kʋ ma.
40028019	A lɛ jũu, yɩ yɔ a wɛr wʋ jaa na yɩ tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ paalsɩ ka ba wa turo ma, na yɩ suoro ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, a Sãa yuor, nɩ a Bie yuor, nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ yuor 'yɔ̃ɔ,
40028020	tɩ na yɩ wile ba ka ba sɔɔ de, tɩ turo bon jaa ɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ. Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka ɩn ma ben a yɩ sɛ̃ sɔ̃ɔ jaa, tɩ tãn a wɛr baarfʋ daar."
41001001	Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ pielfʋ.
41001002	'Yɛ'yɛrɛ kɔ̃ɔ yuor na di Isaiya sɛb naa, "Nyɛ, ɩn tʋ̃ naa a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ka wʋ de nie tɩ chɔɔr a sɔr kʋ fʋ."
41001003	"Kɔkɔr tãna naa a dãlpʋɔ ju, 'Chɔɔr a sɔr kʋ a sɩ Soro na fʋ maal a wʋ sɔr ka wʋ tor.' "
41001004	Lɛ lɛ a Jɔɔn wa, na wʋ wa suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ be a dãlpʋɔ ju, na wʋ mʋɔl 'yɛr, "Yɩ lɩɛb yi a yɩ tɩɛr dɛɛr pɔ so a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ka wʋ vɛ̃ a yelbebe kʋ yɩ."
41001005	Ka a nɩbɛ yire a tẽn ala a jaa na be a Judiya wɛr pɔ, ka a bamɩne mɩ yire a Jerusalɛm. Ba chire naa a ba pʋʋr 'yɛrɛ a ba yelbebe kʋrɔ wʋ tɩchɛ ka wʋ suoro ba jaa a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ a Jordan man pɔ.
41001006	Nyɔɔma kɔɔlʋ fuu lɛ Jɔɔn ma su tɩ de gãn lũn a sɩɛ. Soor nɩ sɩkãa lɛ ɩ a wʋ bʋ̃diir.
41001007	Wʋ 'yɛr naa, "N puor sʋɔ ben be, na wʋ gar ma. A wʋ nafɔɔr mibe gba n ba sɛɛ ɩka n guun for ɛ.
41001008	Maa suoro yɩ naa nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ tɩchɛ 'lɔ na so yɩ naa nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ."
41001009	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ Yesu yi naa Najaretɩ na be a Galilee wɛr pɔ wa, ka a Jɔɔn so wʋ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ a Jordan man pɔ.
41001010	A Yesu na wa yire a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ, wʋ nyɛ naa a saaju na tɔɔ yuo ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wa suro fɩka papa wa kpɛ a Yesu pɔ.
41001011	Tɩ a kɔkɔr yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ 'yɛrɛ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a n binʋ̃nãa, ka a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ma 'maa nɩ fʋ."
41001012	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ de wʋ fɔɔ jaa chiin a dãlpʋɔ ju,
41001013	ka wʋ tɩ be be ber lɩjaayi ka a Satan bɛɛr wʋ kaa. 'Lɔ nɩ a mɔdʋ̃n lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be, ka a malakasɩ wa sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ.
41001014	Jɔɔn ban wa nyɔɔ pɔɔ baar, Yesu chen naa a Galilee na wʋ tɩ mʋɔlɔ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ.
41001015	Wʋ 'yɛr naa, "A sɔ̃ɔ ta naa ka a Nãaŋmɩn di a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ. Yɩ lɩɛb yi a tɩɛr dɛɛr pɔ na yɩ sɔɔ de a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ."
41001016	A lɛ a Yesu na wa de a Galilee man lana, wʋ nyɛ naa Simon nɩ a wʋ yɛbile Andiru ka ba lɔɔrɔ lɔyaar, jɩ̃nyɔɔrbɔ lɛ ba ɩ,
41001017	ka wʋ bʋɔl ba, "Yɩ wa turo ma, ka n lɩɛb yɩ ka yɩ nyɔɔrɔ nɩbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
41001018	Ka ba tɔ̃ɔ tɩɛ a jɩ̃mɛ nyɔɔrfʋ bar tɩ turo wʋ.
41001019	Wʋn wa chen a niem bɩ̃lãa, wʋ nyɛ naa Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn, Jebedee bibiir, a ba be a gboro pɔ chɔɔrɔ a lɔyaarsɩ.
41001020	Wʋn wa nyɛ ba, wʋ bʋɔl ba naa, ka ba bar a ba sãa nɩ a gboro nɩ a bala ban yara tɩ turo a Yesu.
41001021	Be lɛ ba wa chen a Kapenahum ka a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir wa ta, ka a Yesu chen tɩ kpɛ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie tɩ piel wile.
41001022	A nɩbɛ nɛɛr 'maa naa nɩ a wʋ wiilfʋ, bojũu wʋ wile ba naa nɩ Nãaŋmɩn sɔr. Waa ɩ fɩka a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe ɛ.
41001023	A sɩdɛɛr sʋɔ kɔ̃ɔ mɩ chen tɩ kpɛ a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie tãna 'yɛrɛ nɩ,
41001024	"Bãa lɛ a fʋ̃ʋ Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ bʋɔrɔ a sɩ sɛ̃? Fʋ wa naa ɩka fʋ wa sɔ̃ɔ sɩ bar bɩɩ? N bɔ̃ɔ naa a nɩrɛ 'lɔ fʋn ɩ, fʋ ɩ naa a chɛchɛ 'lɔ na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃!"
41001025	Ka a Yesu tãn wʋ, "Pɔɔ a fʋ nɛɛ tɩ wa yi a daba pɔ!"
41001026	Ka a sɩdɛɛr daa a daba lɔb tẽe nɩtãa kpũgul loro tɩ ŋme chɛlma tɩ wa yi a daba pɔ.
41001027	Ka a nɛɛr 'maa a nɩbɛ ka ba lɩɛb sʋrɔ taa, "Bo lɛ? Wiil paal bo mɩ nɩ nyã, na tara kpɛ̃ɔ lɛ! Wʋ ma 'yɛr 'yɛr, ka a sɩdɛbɛ ma tu a wʋ nɛɛ."
41001028	Ka a wʋ yele yaar a Galilee wɛr wʋ jaa.
41001029	Ban wa yi a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie, 'lɔ nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn chen naa a Simon nɩ Andiru yir,
41001030	ka a ɩ̃gãn tɔ a Simon dɩ̃ɛ pɔɔ ka ba 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu.
41001031	Yesu kpɛ naa a wʋ sɛ̃ tɩ nyɔɔ a wʋ nũu sʋ̃ʋ wʋ ka wʋ ir. A ɩ̃gãn tʋl baar wʋ, ka wʋ ir maal bʋ̃diir kʋ ba.
41001032	A jãanʋɔr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa mʋr, a nɩbɛ waan na baalsɩ nɩ a bala a sɩdɛbɛ na tara a Yesu sɛ̃.
41001033	Ka a tẽe nɩbɛ ba jaa wa lɔ̃ɔ a dɔ̃dɔ̃rʋ,
41001034	ka a Yesu sãa nɩyɔɔ na tara baal jaa bʋrɔ. Wʋ mɩ dii naa a sɩdɛbɛ yɔɔ ka a yi, tɩ maa sɔɔ ka a sɩdɛbɛ 'yɛr 'yɛr ɛ, bojũu ba bɔ̃ɔ naa a nɩrɛ 'lɔ wʋn ɩ.
41001035	A wɛr na chaara a bibio pipi tɩ chɛnɛ sɔb, Yesu ir na wʋ yi a yir na wʋ chen a jie ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩka wʋ tɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn.
41001036	Simon nɩ a wʋ taaba mɩ yin bʋɔrɔ wʋ na ba wa nyɛ wʋ,
41001037	na ba 'yɛr, "Nɩbɛ ba jaa yʋɔrɔ na bʋɔrɔ fʋ!"
41001038	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩ ɩ ka sɩ chen jiyuo, a tẽn anyã na gbʋr, ka n tɩ mʋɔl 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr a be, ala 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ n wa."
41001039	Wʋ yɔ naa a Galilee wɛr wʋ jaa na wʋ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie pɔ tɩ na wʋ dire a sɩdɛbɛ mɩ ka a yire.
41001040	Ka a daba ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ na ɩ kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ wa gbur dumo sʋɔr wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ sɔɔ, sãa ma."
41001041	Ka nɩbaal kpɛ a Yesu ka wʋ tur a wʋ nũu sɩɩr a daba tɩ 'yɛr, "N sɔɔ naa. Sa!"
41001042	Ajienaa ka a kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ sa.
41001043	Yesu kpãa wʋ naa kpãkpãan wʋ ɩka,
41001044	"Taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ ɛ. Chen tɩ wiil a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrloro tɩ ir a nɛɛ 'lɔ a Mosesɩ na 'yɛr ka a ɩ dãasɩɛ."
41001045	Tɩchɛ a daba na wa yi wʋ piel naa na wʋ ŋme a Yesu yele yaar, ka a lɛ jũu Yesu ba lɛ tʋ̃ɔ yʋɔrɔ chãa pɔ a tẽe pɔ ɛ. Wʋ ma be naa a tẽe kõkoor, a nɩbɛ chɛnɛ yire jiir jaa waara a wʋ sɛ̃.
41002001	A anyã puor, Yesu lɩɛb wa a Kapenahum, ka nɩbɛ wõ ka wʋ be naa a yir.
41002002	Nɩyɔɔ wan wa duo na ba sɛɛ a die wa tɩ yin a yõo. Ka wa 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋrɔ ba.
41002003	Be lɛ ka daba ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ bɩɛrɛ, a wʋ nuur nɩ a wʋ gbɛɛ kpi naa, ka nɩbɛ anaar jɛ̃jɛl wʋ na ba waan a Yesu sɛ̃.
41002004	Ka ba wa ta, ka jie ba be be a ba na tu kpɛ̃n a be a Yesu na be ɛ, a nɩyɔɔ jũu. Be lɛ ba do a gar ju na ba tɩ ŋmaa puo a jie 'lɔ a Yesu na ara, tɩ na ba de a daba nɩ a fɔbaa 'lɔ ban 'mɔɔn wʋ waan tur bar ka wʋ suu tɩ gã a Yesu niem.
41002005	Be lɛ a Yesu na wa nyɛ a lɛ ban sɔɔ de wʋ, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a dabaala, "N bie, n vɛ̃ naa fʋ yelbebe bar."
41002006	Ka be lɛ ka a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe bamɩne na be be tɩɛrɛ,
41002007	"Ka nyɛ daba na ara fere na wʋ sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn yuor tɛɛ. An lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ nɩrɛ yelbebe vɛ̃ bar, ka Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ?"
41002008	Ajienaa Yesu bɔ̃ɔn naa a lɛ ban tɩɛrɛ a ba pʋʋr pɔ, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Bãa lɛ yɩ tɩɛrɛ a lɛ a yɩ pʋʋr pɔ?
41002009	Buor sʋɔ lɛ ɩ kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃, n 'yɛr ɩka n vɛ̃ naa wʋ yelbebe bar, bɩɩ, n 'yɛr ɩka a daba nyã wʋ ir, 'mɔɔ a wʋ bʋ̃gãnaa, na wʋ kulo nɩ?
41002010	N bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a Nɩsaal Bie tara naa kpɛ̃ɔ a wɛr pɔ na vɛ̃ nɩrɛ yelbebe kʋ wʋ." Be lɛ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba 'lɔ nuur nɩ a gbɛɛ na kpi,
41002011	"Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ, ir, na fʋ 'mɔɔ a bʋ̃gãnaa, na fʋ kulo nɩ."
41002012	Be lɛ, ka wʋ vaa ir 'mɔɔ a bʋ̃gãnaa yin a nɩbɛ ba jaa niem. Nɛɛr 'maa ba naa ka ba dãna Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ, "Saa dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ a lɛ ɛ."
41002013	Yesu lɩɛb chen a man nɛɛ ka nɩyɔɔ wa a wʋ sɛ̃ ka wʋ wile ba.
41002014	A Yesu na wa chiine wʋ nyɛ naa a Alfayasɩ bie, Levi, ka wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a lõpo defʋ jie, ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ir turo ma," ka wʋ ir turo wʋ.
41002015	A lõpodierbe nɩ a yelbetʋ̃nbɔ yɔɔ turo naa a Yesu, ka 'lɔ nɩ a bamɩne nɩ a wʋ poturbo 'mataa dire a Levi yir.
41002016	A Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe na ɩ a Faraseemɩne nyɛ a lɛ wʋn jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a lõpodierbe nɩ a yelbetʋ̃nbɔ 'mataa dire, ka ba sʋʋr a wʋ poturbo, "Bãa lɛ so a daba nyã na 'mataa dire nɩ a lõpodierbe nɩ a yelbetʋ̃nbɔ?"
41002017	Yesu wõ naa a lɛ ban 'yɛr, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩrɛ na kpɛ̃mɛ waa chiine tɩtɩlɛ jie ɛ. Baalaa lɛ ma chen. N ba wa ɩka n wa bʋɔl a nɩtorsɩ ɛ. N wa naa ɩka n wa bʋɔl a yelbebe tʋ̃nbɔ ka ba wa lɩɛb a tɩɛr."
41002018	Jɔɔn poturbo nɩ a Faraseemɩne nɩbɛ gal kɔ̃, ka nɩbɛ wa sʋʋr a Yesu, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a Jɔɔn poturbo nɩ a Farasee poturbo ma gal kɔ̃, tɩchɛ ka a fʋ̃ʋ poturbo maa gal kɔ̃ ɛ?"
41002019	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an ɩ ka nɩbɛ be a pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ jie tɩ tʋ̃ɔ kɔ̃ gal? Wʋn chɛnɛ be a ba sɛ̃, ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
41002020	A daar 'lɔ ban wa de a pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ, ban gal a kɔ̃.
41002021	"Nɩrɛ maa ŋmaa fɔpaalaa sɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ fɔkoraa pɔ ɛ. 'Lɔ be sɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a lɛ, a fɔpaalaa na tɔɔ naa a fɔkoraa chɩɛr.
41002022	Nɩrɛ maa de dãbɩ̃ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ wɔkoraa pɔ ɛ. 'Lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ, a wʋɔ na pur naa, ka a dãa nɩ a wʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ. Wʋ ma 'yɔ̃ɔ naa dãbɩ̃ɩn wɔpaalaa pɔ."
41002023	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar, Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo kpɛ̃n tala puo sãlsɔɔ, ka a wʋ poturbo piel fɔrɔ a bʋ̃bie.
41002024	Ka a Faraseemɩne 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Nyɛ lɛ a fʋ poturbo na ɩrɛ. Bo lɛ so ka ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir? A ba tara sɔr ɛ."
41002025	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yaa bɔ̃ɔ a par a lɛ yɩn kar kaa a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ a nãa David nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ na ba dɔ̃ɔ tara bon na di ɛ!
41002026	A ber ala pɔ Abiyata lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, kɔ̃ dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ ba, ka wʋ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn yir, ka a Abiyata de a paanʋ̃ɔ ala ban bin kʋ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ wʋ, ka wʋ 'wɔb. A paanʋ̃ɔ ala a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlorbo tɛɛ lɛ ma 'wɔb, a ba tara sɔr ɩka nɩyuo wʋ 'wɔb ɛ, tɩchɛ ka David 'wɔb tɩ de kʋ a bala na be a wʋ sɛ̃, ka ba mɩ 'wɔb."
41002027	Be lɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir ben be a nɩbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ, a ba ɩ a nɩbɛ ben be a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
41002028	Ala lɛ so ka a Nɩsaal Bie ɩ a Soro lɔ̃ɔn a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir gba."
41003001	Sɔ̃ɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ go Yesu chen tɩ kpɛ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie, ka a daba kɔ̃ɔ mɩ be be ka a wʋ nũpɛl kpi.
41003002	Ka a nɩbɛ bamɩne na be be bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba gar a Yesu, be lɛ ba tɔɔ gbʋr kaara wʋ. Ka wʋn sãa naa a daba nũu baal a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir bɩɩ.
41003003	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a daba nũpɛl na kpi, "Ir ara a sɩ jaa nyɛ fʋ."
41003004	Be lɛ ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Tʋ̃buor sʋɔ lɛ tara sɔr a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir daar ɩka fʋ tʋ̃, a fʋ maal vɩla bɩɩ dɛɛr, fʋ faa nyɛvʋr bɩɩ fʋ kʋ wʋ?" Ka ba ɩ jaa gbulo gbulo.
41003005	Wʋ kaa naa ba jaa gʋɔr nɩ suur, ka a wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ a ba bachɛlfʋ jũu. Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba 'lɔ nũpɛl na kpi, "Tur a fʋ nũu." Wʋ tur naa ka a nũpɛl wʋ jaa sa.
41003006	Be lɛ ka a Faraseemɩne yi chen a Hɛrɔd nɩbɛ sɛ̃, a ba tɩ 'mataa guoro a Yesu, bʋɔrɔ sɔr 'lɔ ban na tu kʋ wʋ.
41003007	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo yin chen a man pɔ ka a nɩyɔɔ na yi Galilee wɛr tu ba.
41003008	Nɩyɔyɔɔ mɩ yi naa Judiya wɛr, Jerusalɛm, Idumea wɛr nɩ a Jordan man gɔ̃ɔn, nɩ a tẽn na be Tire nɩ Sidon wɛr pɔ, wa a wʋ sɛ̃ bojũu ba wõ naa a lɛ jaa wʋn tʋ̃.
41003009	A nɩyɔɔ jũu, Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "Yɩ kaa nyɛ gboro kʋ ma ka n sɛr bɩ̃lãa." Wʋ 'yɛr naa a lɛ bojũu waa bʋɔrɔ ɩka a nɩbɛ ba mɩl pɔɔ wʋ ɛ.
41003010	A nɩbɛ yɔɔ wʋn sãa lɛ so, a baalsɩ dara taa bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba sɩɩr wʋ.
41003011	A sɩdɛbɛ na ma wa nyɛ a Yesu ba ma da naa a nɩrɛ 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ ban be lɔb tẽe tɩ tãna 'yɛrɛ nɩ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie!"
41003012	Tɩchɛ wʋ kpaal ban jũu, ka ba taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ wʋn ɩ ɛ.
41003013	Yesu do naa a tɔ̃ɔ ju tɩ bʋɔl a bala wʋn bʋɔrɔ ka ba do wa a wʋ sɛ̃.
41003014	A ba pɔ lɛ wʋ kaa ir pie nɩ ayi, bʋɔlɔ ba nɩtʋ̃nsɩ, ka ba na be a wʋ sɛ̃, ka wʋ ma tʋ̃ ba ka ba chen tɩ mʋɔl 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr,
41003015	tɩ tara kpɛ̃ɔ dire nɩ sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire.
41003016	A nɩbɛ pie nɩ ayi bala wʋn ir yoe lɛ a anyã. Simon, wʋn lɛ kʋ wʋ yopaalaa Pita.
41003017	Jemesɩ, nɩ a wʋ yɛbile Jɔɔn, a ba sãa yuor lɛ Jebedee, wʋ bʋɔlɔ ba naa Bɔɔnɛgasɩ, a par lɛ sa tãna bibiir.
41003018	Andiru, Filip, Batolomi, Matiu, Tomasɩ, Jemesɩ na ɩ Alfayasɩ bidaba, Tadius, Simon na mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a wʋ wɛr yele,
41003019	nɩ a Judas Isɩkariyot, 'lɔ lɛ na wa de a Yesu tɩr.
41003020	A Yesu na lɩɛb wa a yir, nɩyɔɔ wa naa wa lɔ̃ɔ go, ka 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ poturbo ba tara jaa gba na di ɛ.
41003021	Be lɛ a wʋ yir dẽme na wa wõ a lɛ, ba chen naa ɩka ba tɩ ka wʋ, bojũu ba 'yɛr naa ɩka, "Burbur kpɛ wʋ naa."
41003022	Ka a Mosesɩ Nɛɛr wiwiilbe bamɩne na yi a Jerusalɛm mɩ 'yɛrɛ, "A Beeljebul, lɛ pɔb wʋ! A sɩdɛbɛ nãa lɛ wʋ ma de dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire."
41003023	Yesu bʋɔl naa a nɩbɛ na wʋ lɔb sʋkpar kʋ ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a Satan na ɩ lɛ dii a Satan?
41003024	Ala ɩ nãa ir jɛɛrɛ nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nãalʋ̃ʋ, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ wʋn ɩ ara?
41003025	Yir nɩbɛ mɩ ir jɛɛrɛ taa, a yir 'lɔ nɩbɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'mataa kpɛ ɛ.
41003026	Ala ɩ a Satan ir naa na wʋ jɛɛrɛ nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, wʋ mɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ara ɛ, a wʋ baaraa lɛ.
41003027	Yelmɩ̃ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ gãdaa yir tɩ ju a wʋ bonsɩ ka waa de nie lũ wʋ ɛ. 'Lɔ wa lũ wʋ a lɛ wa baar, wʋn pãa tʋ̃ɔ naa a wʋ yir bonsɩ ju.
41003028	Sɩrɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yeldɛbɛ nɩ ferfʋ a jaa nɩbɛ na fere sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn yuor ban nyɛn vɛ̃ kʋfʋ.
41003029	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na fere nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋ̃ nyɛ vɛ̃ kʋfʋ ɛ, bojũu wʋ lo naa a yeldɛɛr 'lɔ pɔ, na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ."
41003030	Ban 'yɛr ɩka wʋ tara naa a sɩdɛɛr lɛ so ka wʋ 'yɛr a lɛ.
41003031	Be lɛ ka a Yesu ma nɩ a wʋ yɛɛr wa. Ba ara naa a yõo tɩ tʋ̃ nɩrɛ ka wʋ bʋɔl wʋ.
41003032	Nɩyɔɔ jɩ̃nɛ naa jilʋ̃ a Yesu tɩ ba 'yɛr wʋ, "A fʋ ma nɩ a fʋ yɛɛr be naa a yõo bʋɔrɔ fʋ."
41003033	Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "An lɛ ɩ a n ma nɩ a n yɛɛr?"
41003034	Be lɛ wʋ kaa a bala na jɩ̃nɛ jilʋ̃ wʋ tɩ 'yɛr, "Banyã lɛ ɩ a n ma nɩ a n yɛɛr!
41003035	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na turo a Nãaŋmɩn sɔr, 'lɔ lɛ a n yɛbɛ nɩ a n yɛpɔɔ nɩ a n ma."
41004001	Sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ go, Yesu piel wile a man nɛɛ. A nɩyɔyɔɔ na wa lɔ̃ɔ jũu, wʋ kpɛ naa a gboro pɔ jɩ̃nɛ, tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ ara kɔɔ a kʋ̃ɔ nɛɛ.
41004002	Sʋkpar lɛ wʋ lɔɔrɔ wile nɩ ba yelyɔɔ, sʋkpa ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩ nyã:
41004003	"Yɩ chɛlɛ! Kʋɔraa lɛ yi chen ɩka wʋ tɩ yaar a wʋ bʋ̃bʋrɔ.
41004004	Wʋ yaar naa ka amɩne lo a sɔr pɔ ka a lubil wa tuur di.
41004005	Ka amɩne mɩ lo a jie 'lɔ a kʋsɩbɛ na waa gar a tãna, na a bul fɔɔ, a tãna na ba tɩrɛ jũu.
41004006	Tɩchɛ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa nyãa, a jʋɔl naa na a kpi, bojũu a ba tara nyɩbɛ ɛ.
41004007	Amɩne mɩ tɩ lo naa gʋʋr pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a gʋʋr bul fɩ̃ɩn naa tara, a ba tʋ̃ɔ dɔɔ ɛ.
41004008	Ka amɩne mɩ tɩ lo a kɔjɔ̃ vɩla pɔ, na a dɔɔ yɔɔ. Ka amɩne dɔɔ a lɩjɛr nɩ pie, amɩne lɩjaata ka amɩne mɩ kɔbaa."
41004009	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩrɛ jaa na tara toor, wʋ chɛlɛ!"
41004010	A nɩyɔyɔɔ bala na wa chen tɩ chɛ a nɩbɛ bala na turo wʋ nɩ a wʋ poturbo pie nɩ a ayi bala wʋn ir, ka a ba sʋʋr wʋ a sʋkpar par.
41004011	Be lɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn 'lɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ yɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ yelsɔɔlaa, tɩchɛ a banyã 'lɔ na ba pʋɔ ɛ, a yelsɩ a jaa ɩ naa sʋkpar kʋ ba.
41004012	A lɛ jũu, 'Ba ma kãan lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ ba maa nyɛ ɛ, na ba ma chɛl lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ ba maa wõ ɛ. Ala ba ɩ lɛ ɛ ban lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr ka Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃ kʋ ba.' "
41004013	Ka Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Yaa bɔ̃ɔ a sʋkpa nyã par ɛ? Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩn ɩ wa bɔ̃ɔ sʋkpa jaa par?
41004014	Yɩ kaa, a kʋɔraa lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na yaara a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr.
41004015	Nɩbɛ bamɩne kaara naa fɩka a bʋ̃bie ala ban yaar ka a lo a sɔr pɔ. Bala wa wõ a 'yɛr wa baar, a Satan ma wa naa, wa de a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbir ban bʋr a ba nyãa pɔ.
41004016	Ala mɩ na lo a jie 'lɔ a kʋsɩbɛ na waa gar a tãna ɩ naa a bala na wõ a 'yɛr na ba ma sɔɔ de fɔɔ jaa nɩ pʋpɛl,
41004017	tɩchɛ baa tara nyɩbɛ ɛ, ba maa kor ɛ. A 'yɛr jũu, wõm bɩɩ gefʋ wa wa a ba sɛ̃, ba ma lɩɛb puor fɔɔ jaa.
41004018	A ala mɩ na lo a gʋʋr pɔ ɩ naa a bala na wõ a 'yɛr,
41004019	tɩchɛ ka a ɩ̃gãn nyã wõm, nɩ a bʋ̃tarsɩ bɛlfʋ, nɩ a bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ fɩ̃ɩn a 'yɛr, ka waa tʋ̃ɔ dɔɔ ɛ.
41004020	A anyã mɩ na lo a kɔjɔ̃ pɔ ɩ naa a bala na wõ a 'yɛr na ba sɔɔ de na ba dɔɔ jur, ka amɩne ɩ lɩjɛr nɩ pie, amɩne lɩjaata, amɩne mɩ kɔbaa."
41004021	Wʋ sʋʋr ba naa, "Ba ma chʋm fɩ̃tɩn na ba de laa kpa pɔɔ bɩɩ de su gado pĩlem bɩɩ? A ba ɩ a jie 'lɔ wʋn na chaar nɩrɛ jaa lɛ ba ma dɔɔl ɛ?
41004022	Bon jaa na pɔɔ ban yuo wʋ naa, ka ala a jaa mɩ na sɔɔl yi chãa pɔ.
41004023	Nɩrɛ jaa na tara toor, wʋ chɛlɛ!"
41004024	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔ chɛlɛ sʋ̃ a lɛ yɩn wõnõ. A lɛ fʋn man tɩr, lɛ mɩ lɛ ban man kʋ fʋ, tɩ dɔɔl gba.
41004025	Nɩrɛ jaa na tara, Nãaŋmɩn ma vɛ̃ naa ka wʋ nyɛrɛ dɔɔlɔ, nɩrɛ nyã mɩ na ba tara ɛ, a bɩ̃lãa ala gba wʋn tara, Nãaŋmɩn na de naa a wʋ sɛ̃."
41004026	Tɩ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nɩtɔ̃ lɛ wʋ kaara. Daba ma yaar a wʋ bʋ̃bʋrɔ bar.
41004027	Tɩ̃sɔɔ nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ, ka wʋ gãn bɩɩ wʋ ir naa, a bʋ̃bie ma bulaa naa nʋ̃ɔ, tɩchɛ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ gba maa bɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
41004028	A bʋ̃bie ma bul naa a tẽe naa tɔ vaar tɩ dɔɔ jur, bɩ a bie.
41004029	Ala wa bɩ baar, wʋ ma chiin nɩ sʋɔ tɩ ŋman bojũu a ŋmab sɔ̃ɔ ta naa."
41004030	Ka Yesu lɛ 'yɛr, "Bo lɛ sɩn de man a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ bɩɩ sʋkpa buor lɛ sɩn lɔb gbɛb wʋ?
41004031	Wʋ kaara fɩka a kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ bir, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a bʋ̃bie a jaa pɔ bʋ̃bile.
41004032	Tɩchɛ wʋ ma bul ɩ tɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wʋ tɛ wilbɛrɛ, ka a lubil ma wa mara a wʋ 'maar pɔ."
41004033	Yesu de naa sʋkpayɔɔ na nyɛtaa na wʋ 'yɛr a 'yɛr kʋ ba, a lɛ an na ɩ ka ba tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a par.
41004034	Sʋkpar tɛɛ lɛ wʋ ma de 'yɛrɛ nɩ a 'yɛr kʋrɔ ba. Tɩchɛ ala wa ɩ 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ poturbo tɛɛ lɛ, wʋ ma wiil naa a jaa par kʋ ba.
41004035	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ jãanʋɔr, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "Yɩ ɩ a sɩ gɔ̃ɔ chen a man gɔ̃ɔn."
41004036	Ba bar naa a nɩyɔyɔɔ bala tɩchɛ ka a wʋ poturbo tara wʋ, ka ba 'matãan a gborsɩ amɩne gɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
41004037	Ka a man kʋ̃ɔ sɛkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ ire ka a kʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a gboro pɔ ɩrɛ na sɛɛ
41004038	tɩchɛ ka a Yesu be a gboro par gã kɔɔl wʋ ju guro. Ka a wʋ poturbo sɩ̃ɩ wʋ na ba sʋrɔ wʋ, "Wiwile, a ba bã fʋ sɩn mʋrɔ bɩɩ?"
41004039	Be lɛ ka wʋ ir tãn a sɛsɛbɛ nɩ a man, "Yɩ ŋmaa vʋʋr! Yɩ ara a lɛ nɛ!" Ka a sɛsɛbɛ ŋmaa vʋʋr ka a man ara jomm.
41004040	Ka wʋ sʋʋr a wʋ poturbo, "Bo lɛ so ka yɩ joro a dãbɩ̃ɛ? Yɩ chɛnɛ na ba sɔɔ ma bɩɩ?"
41004041	Ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba ka ba lɩɛb sʋrɔ taa, "An lɛ a nyã ka a sɛsɛbɛ nɩ a man tu a wʋ nɛɛ?"
41005001	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo gɔ̃ɔ naa a man, a Gerasenɩ nɩbɛ wɛr pɔ.
41005002	Yesu na wa yi a gboro pɔ, daba na gele yi naa a yar par wa tuor wʋ.
41005003	A gẽgelaa nyã kpɩɛrɛ naa a yar par ka nɩrɛ jaa ba be be na tʋ̃ɔ lũ wʋ nɩ bɔ̃jɔrsɩ gba ɛ.
41005004	Ba ma lũ naa a wʋ gbɛɛ nɩ a nuur tɩchɛ ka wʋ ŋma, tɩ kar a kue ala bar. Nɩrɛ jaa ba be be na tʋ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ.
41005005	Tɩ̃sɔɔ nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ, wʋ ma be naa a yar par nɩ a tɔ̃n ju tãna tɩ ŋmara a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ kʋsɩbɛ.
41005006	Wʋn wa nyɛ a Yesu na be tɛɛr, wʋ jo naa tɩ lo gbur dumo a wʋ niem,
41005007	tɩ na wʋ ŋme chɛlma 'yɛrɛ, "Bo fʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka fʋ ɩ ma? Fʋ ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na gar a jaa Bie pɔn Nãaŋmɩn ɩka fʋ kʋ̃ ge ma ɛ."
41005008	Bojũu Yesu dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ wʋ ɩka, "A fʋ̃ʋ sɩdɛɛr wa yi a daba pɔ."
41005009	Be lɛ ka Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Bãa a fʋ yuor di?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Sɩyɔɔ, bojũu sɩ waa naa."
41005010	Ka wʋ sʋɔr a Yesu yãayãabɩlɛ ɩka wʋ ta dii wʋ bar a jie 'lɔ ɛ.
41005011	Doyɔɔ mɩ ara na gbʋr a tɔ̃ɔ, dire.
41005012	Ka a sɩdɛbɛ sʋɔr a Yesu, "Ir sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a dor ala pɔ na fʋ sɔɔ ka sɩ tɩ kpɛ a ba pɔ."
41005013	Wʋ sɔɔ naa ka a sɩdɛbɛ yi tɩ kpɛ a dor ala. A ɩ naa dor tur ayi (2,000) ka a jaa tĩgbil suu tɩ kpɛ a man pɔ gbʋ̃m kpi kpi.
41005014	A bala na kaara a dor jon kul a tẽe pɔ nɩ a tẽbil ala na gbʋr tɩ 'yɛr a lɛ na ɩ. Ka a nɩbɛ yi chen ɩka ba tɩ kaa.
41005015	Ba wa naa a Yesu sɛ̃ wa nyɛ a daba 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ tara a sɩdɛyɔɔ gele ka wʋ chɩ su bonsɩ jɩ̃nɛ, ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba.
41005016	A bala na nyɛ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ a lɛ na ɩ a daba na dɔ̃ɔ tara a sɩdɛbɛ nɩ a dor 'yɛr,
41005017	ka a nɩbɛ piel sʋɔrɔ a Yesu ka wʋ yi a ba wɛr pɔ.
41005018	Yesu na wa kpɩɛrɛ a gboro pɔ ka a daba 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩdɛbɛ na yi sʋɔr wʋ ɩka wʋ ɩ a ba 'mataa chen.
41005019	Ka a Yesu ba sɔɔ ɛ, tɩ 'yɛr wʋ, "Kul a fʋ yir dẽme sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba a lɛ a Soro na ɩ kʋ fʋ, nɩ a lɛ wʋn jo a fʋ nɩbaal."
41005020	A daba chen na wʋ tɩ piel 'yɛrɛ a lɛ a Yesu na maal kʋ wʋ a wɛr 'lɔ pɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Dekapolisɩ. Ka a nɛɛr 'maa a nɩbɛ.
41005021	Yesu na wa gɔ̃ɔ a man gɔ̃ɔn go, nɩyɔyɔɔ lɔ̃ɔ naa na ba jilʋ̃ wʋ. Wʋ chɛnɛ na ara a man nɛɛ,
41005022	ka a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Jairusɩ wa a be. Wʋn wa nyɛ a Yesu,
41005023	wʋ gbur dumo a Yesu niem tɩ sʋɔr wʋ, "Yãayãabɩlɛ, a n bipɔɔbile lɛ ɩ baal ɩrɛ na kpi. Wa dɔɔl wʋ a fʋ nũu ka wʋ sa ta kpi ɛ."
41005024	Ka a Yesu nɩ a daba 'mataa chiine. Nɩyɔyɔɔ turo naa dara taa tɩɛrɛ wʋ.
41005025	Pɔɔ kɔ̃ɔ mɩ ben be lo sɩɛ suoro faara yuomo pie nɩ ayi.
41005026	Wʋ bal di dɔɔyɛ yɔɔ a tɩtɩɩlbɛ jie na wʋ sɔ̃ɔ bon jaa wʋn tara tɩ ba sa ɛ. Ka a baal tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ.
41005027	Wʋn wa wõ a Yesu yele, wʋ tu naa a puor tɩ sɩɩr a wʋ fuu,
41005028	bojũu wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ. "Maa tʋ̃ɔ sɩɩr a wʋ fuu gba, ɩn sa naa, na n pɛ̃n."
41005029	Wʋn wa sɩɩr a Yesu fuu nɛɛ wa baar, a jɩ̃ɩ ŋmaa naa a dẽdẽe daa ka wʋ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a wʋ wʋʋr baar naa.
41005030	Ka a Yesu mɩ bɔ̃ɔn a fɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a kpɛ̃ɔ na yi a wʋ sɛ̃. Ka a wʋ lɩɛb a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ sʋʋr, "An lɛ sɩɩr a n fuu?"
41005031	Ka a wʋ poturbo 'yɛr, "Nyɛ a lɛ a nɩyɔyɔɔ banyã na dara taa tɩɛrɛ fʋ, tɩchɛ a fʋ sʋrɔ a sʋɔ 'lɔ na sɩɩr fʋ!"
41005032	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu chɛnɛ kaara gʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ nyɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɩɩr wʋ.
41005033	Ka a pɔɔ na bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ na ɩ, dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ wʋ naa ka wʋ mɩrɛ na wʋ wa gbur dumo a Yesu niem tɩ 'yɛr a lɛ jaa na ɩ.
41005034	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N yɛpɔɔ, fʋn sɔɔ ma jũu, fʋ sa naa. Kulo nɩ ɩ̃gãn 'maar, a fʋ dɔɔyɛ baar naa."
41005035	A Yesu ba 'yɛr baar ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩbɛ kɔ̃ɔ yi a Jairusɩ yir wa 'yɛr wʋ, "A fʋ bie kpi naa. Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wiwile go?"
41005036	Yesu ba chɛlɛ a lɛ ban 'yɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba, "Taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Sɔɔ ma dɛ."
41005037	Yesu ba sɔɔ ka nɩrɛ jaa tu wʋ ɛ, ka Pita nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ a wʋ yɛbile Jɔɔn tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
41005038	Ban wa ta a Jairusɩ yir, Yesu nyɛ naa a nɩbɛ na kõnõ ŋmiere chɛlsɩ.
41005039	Ka wʋ kpɛ tɩ sʋʋr ba, "Bãa lɛ yɩ kõnõ ŋmiere nɩ a chɛlsɩ a lɛ? A bie ba kpi ɛ. Wʋ gur naa."
41005040	A ba laara tʋrɔ nɩ wʋ. Wʋ dii naa a nɩbɛ ba jaa bar ka ba yi tɩ wʋ tara a bie sãa nɩ a ma nɩ a wʋ poturbo bala wʋn 'mataa chiin, a ba kpɛ a jie 'lɔ a bikũu na be.
41005041	Ka wʋ tɩ nyɔɔ a pɔɔbile nũu tɩ 'yɛr, "Talita kum!" A par lɛ a Yesu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr pɔ, "Pɔɔbile, ir!"
41005042	Ka wʋ vaa ir chiine. Yuomo pie nɩ ayi bie lɛ. Ka a yele 'maa ba nɛɛ.
41005043	Yesu kpaal ba naa jũu ka ba taa vɛ̃ ka a nɩrɛ jaa wõ naa ɛ. Tɩ 'yɛr ɩka ba kʋ a pɔɔbile bʋ̃diir ka wʋ di.
41006001	Yesu yi naa a be ka a wʋ poturbo tu wʋ ka a ba 'mataa kul a Najaretɩ na ɩ a wʋ tẽe.
41006002	Ka a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir wa ta, ka wʋ kpɛ be a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie tɩ piel wile, ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na wõ nɛɛr 'maa. Ka ba sʋrɔ, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ a daba nyã nyɛ a bɔ̃ɔfʋ nyã? Yɛ̃ buor lɛ a nyã wʋn tara na wʋ gba tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃?
41006003	A ba ɩ a mɩmɩɛrɛ lɛ ɛ? A ba ɩ a Mɛɛr bie lɛ ɛ, a wʋ yɛbil ɩ Jemesɩ nɩ Josesɩ nɩ Judas nɩ Simon ɛ? Ka a wʋ yɛpɔbɔ mɩ be ka a sɩ sɛ̃ ɛ?"
41006004	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ nyɛrɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ jie jaa, tɩchɛ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tẽe nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ sɛ̃ lɛ waa nyɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ ɛ."
41006005	Waa tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ yɔɔ a be ɛ, tɩ wʋ dɔɔl a wʋ nũu baalsɩ bɩ̃lãa a ba sa.
41006006	Yesu nɛɛ 'maa wʋ naa bojũu baa sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ. Wʋ yɔn gʋɔr a tẽn na wʋ wile.
41006007	Wʋ bʋɔl naa a wʋ poturbo Pie nɩ Ayi bala wʋn dɔ̃ɔ ir, ka ba wa a wʋ sɛ̃ ka wʋ tʋ̃ ba ayir yir, na wʋ kʋ ba kpɛ̃ɔ ka ba tʋ̃ɔ sɩdɛbɛ.
41006008	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ta de bon jaa ɛ, yɩ tara dadiirsɩ tɛɛ. Yɩ ta tara bʋ̃diir ɛ, bɩɩ wʋʋr ɛ, bɩɩ yɔ̃ɔ libie a yɩ sɩɩr gãma pɔ ɛ.
41006009	Yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ su nafɔbɔ nɩ fuu bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ.
41006010	Yir jaa pɔ yɩn wa kpɛ, yɩ be a be tɩ ta a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ yɩn wa yi a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ.
41006011	Tẽe jaa pɔ yɩn wa kpɛ ka baa de yɩ ɛ, bɩɩ sɔɔ a 'yɛr ɛ, yɩn wa yire yɩ kpoor a yɩ gbɛɛ tã-uul ka a di a ba dɛɛr dãasɩɛ."
41006012	Ba yin chen tɩ mʋɔlɔ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɩka a nɩbɛ ba lɩɛb ba tɩɛr.
41006013	Ba diin a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi, tɩ 'lɩɩ baalsɩ kãa ka ba sa.
41006014	A nãa Hɛrɔd mɩ wõ naa a anyã, bojũu nɩrɛ jaa wõ naa a Yesu yuor. Ka a bamɩne 'yɛrɛ, "A Jɔɔn 'lɔ na ɩ a kɔ̃suoro, 'lɔ lɛ tɔ̃ɔ yi a yaa pɔ, ala lɛ so ka wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ a lɛ."
41006015	Ka a banyã mɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Elaija lɛ." Ka a bamɩne mɩ chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ, "Wʋ ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩtãa a bala na dɔ̃ɔ be be a kõro jaa."
41006016	Tɩchɛ a Hɛrɔd na wa wõ, wʋ 'yɛr naa, "A Jɔɔn 'lɔ ɩn vɛ̃ ka ba ŋmaa a wʋ ju lɛ, yi."
41006017	A Hɛrɔd mɩ̃ɛ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka ba nyɔɔ a Jɔɔn waan, wa lũ 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ. Wʋ ɩ naa a nɩtɔ̃, a wʋ yɛbile Filip pɔɔ Hɛrɔdiyas wʋn de jũu.
41006018	Jɔɔn 'yɛr kʋ a Hɛrɔd, "A ba tara sɔr ɩka fʋ de a fʋ yɛbil vʋr pɔɔ kul ɛ."
41006019	Ka a Hɛrɔdiyas tara nɩ a Jɔɔn jɛɛr bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ kʋ wʋ, tɩchɛ waa tʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
41006020	A Hɛrɔd bɔ̃ɔ naa a Jɔɔn na ɩ nɩsʋ̃ nɩ chɛchɛ, na wʋ joro a Jɔɔn dãbɩ̃ɛ, na wʋ gu wʋ tara. A Hɛrɔd wa wõ a Jɔɔn 'yɛr a ma sɔb wʋn nɩbir, tɩchɛ wʋ ma bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ chɛlɛ a wʋ 'yɛr.
41006021	Tɩchɛ sɔr wa yuon kʋ a Hɛrɔdiyas a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a nãa na wa maala a wʋ dɔɔfʋ bɩbir yele. A wʋ dɔɔfʋ bɩbir nyãna daar, wʋ bʋɔl naa a nɩbɛrɛ bala na turo a wʋ puor, nɩ a sojasɩ nɩbɛrɛ, nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ na be a Galilee pɔ.
41006022	A Hɛrɔdiyas bipɔɔ wa kpɛ naa, na wʋ sɛ a bɩ̃nɛ ka a pɛl a nãa Hɛrɔd nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛrɛ bala ba jaa pʋɔ. Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a pɔɔbile, "Sʋɔr ma bon jaa fʋn bʋɔrɔ, ɩn kʋ fʋ naa."
41006023	Be lɛ wʋ põl kʋ a pɔɔbile, "Bon jaa fʋn sʋɔr ala ɩ a n nãalʋ̃ʋ ŋmaa gba lɛ, n na kʋ fʋ naa."
41006024	Ka wʋ yi chen tɩ sʋʋr a wʋ ma, "Bo lɛ ɩn sʋɔr?" Ka a wʋ ma 'yɛr wʋ, "Tɩ sʋɔr a Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suor ju."
41006025	Ka a pɔɔbile yi pɔɔ fɔɔ lɛ kpɛ a nãa sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "N bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Jɔɔn Kɔ̃suor ju a la'yɛlma pɔ kʋ ma a pʋ̃pãanyã."
41006026	A nãa pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa, tɩchɛ a nɩbɛ bala wʋn bʋɔl na wʋn põl kʋ a pɔɔbile jũu, waa bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ tɔr ɛ.
41006027	Ka wʋ tʋ̃ a nɩkʋrɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ a dẽdẽe daa ɩka wʋ chen tɩ ŋmaa a Jɔɔn ju waan. A daba chen tɩ ŋmaa a Jɔɔn ju a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ
41006028	'yɔ̃ɔ a la'yɛlma pɔ waan, wa kʋ a pɔɔbile ka wʋ de kʋ a wʋ ma.
41006029	A Jɔɔn poturbo na wõ a lɛ, ba chen tɩ 'mɔɔ wʋ na ba ũu.
41006030	A Yesu nɩtʋ̃nsɩ lɩɛb wa lɔ̃ɔ taa a wʋ sɛ̃, na ba wa man a lɛ jaa ban tʋ̃ tɩ wiil a nɩbɛ, na ba kʋ a Yesu.
41006031	A nɩbɛ yɔɔ na waara tɩ chiine jũu, jaa gba ba be be a ban di ɛ. Be lɛ ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ wa a sɩn tɛɛ chen a jie 'lɔ a nɩbɛ na ba be ɛ, a yɩ tɩ jɩ̃nɛ pɛ̃n."
41006032	Ba kpɛ naa a gboro bala tɛɛ chen a jie 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
41006033	Tɩchɛ a nɩbɛ na wa nyɛ ban chiine ba bɔ̃ɔ ba naa. A ba yi a tẽn a jaa de nie jon gbɛɛ tɩ ara a be.
41006034	A Yesu na wa tɩ ta, na wʋ nyɛ a nɩyɔɔ a ba ɩrɛ nɩbaal a wʋ sɛ̃, ban kaara fɩka piir na ba tara chɩnɛ jũu, wʋ piel wile ba yelyɔɔ.
41006035	Mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa mʋrɔ a wʋ poturbo wa naa wa 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "A ka ɩ naa mɔgɔ̃ɔ, tɩ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ mɩ mʋrɔ;
41006036	wɛl a nɩbɛ bar a ba chen a por nɩ a tẽn na gbʋr tɩ bɔ bʋ̃diir da di."
41006037	Ka be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr sɔɔ ba, "Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ yɩ kʋ ba bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ a ba di." Ka a poturbo 'yɛr ɩka, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ sɩn nyɛ a libie anyãna? Nɩbʋ̃'yen ŋmɛrsɩ aniin sãyar gba! Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ sɩn ɩ kʋ ba jaa bʋ̃diir?"
41006038	A be lɛ a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Paanʋ̃ɔsɩ aŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tara? Yɩ chen tɩ kaa." Be lɛ ba chen tɩ kaa tɩ wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu, nɩ jɩ̃mɛ ayi."
41006039	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo a ba ɩ a nɩbɛ ba jaa a ba jɛ̃ gbulsɩ a mɔ'yɔlɔ ju.
41006040	Be lɛ a nɩbɛ jɩ̃nɛ jɩ̃nɛ, a gbulsɩ gbulsɩ. Bamɩne jɩ̃nɛ naa kɔɔr kɔɔr, ka bamɩne mɩ jɩ̃nɛ lɩjaayi nɩ piir.
41006041	A Yesu de naa a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu nɩ a jɩ̃mɛ ayi ala na wʋ kaa saaju tɩ dʋl puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan. Wʋ de naa a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ ŋma ŋma tɩ de kʋ a wʋ poturbo tɩ 'yɛr, "Yɩ de põ a nɩbɛ." Tɩ lɛ de a jɩ̃mɛ ayi ala mɩ ŋma põ a nɩbɛ.
41006042	A nɩbɛ ba jaa din, na ba tɩɩ,
41006043	tɩchɛ ka a poturbo wob a bʋ̃ŋmaara 'yɔ̃ɔ pɛr pie nɩ ayi.
41006044	A nɩbɛ bala na dɔ̃ɔ di a bʋ̃diir ala, dɔɔr tɛɛ ɩ naa tur anũu.
41006045	Ajienaa, ka a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ poturbo a ba kpɛ a gboro na ba de nie chiine a Betɩsaida tɩ wʋ na wɛl a nɩbɛ bar.
41006046	Wʋn wa bar ba wa baar, wʋ do naa a tɔ̃ɔ ju ɩka wʋ tɩ puor.
41006047	A wɛr na wa sɔɔrɔ, a gboro be naa a man sãlsɔɔ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ be a wɛyõo, 'lɔ tɛɛ.
41006048	Wʋ nyɛ naa a wʋ poturbo ka ba mɔ̃nɔ̃ a gboro faara bojũu a sɛsɛbɛ furo na tuoro ba. A wɛr na wa gbʋrɔ a chaarfʋ, wʋ yin chiine a kʋ̃ɔ ju waara a ba sɛ̃, ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ po ba.
41006049	Ban wa nyɛ wʋn chiine a kʋ̃ɔ ju a lɛ, ba tɩɛr ɩka kpĩin lɛ, na ba ŋme chɛlsɩ,
41006050	bojũu ba jaa nyɛ wʋ naa ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba. Ajienaa, ka a Yesu tãn, "Yɩ nyɔɔ nyãa! Maa lɛ! Yɩ taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ."
41006051	Tɩ pãa kpɛ a gboro pɔ ka a sɛsɛbɛ ŋmaa vʋʋr. Ka a nɛɛr 'maa ba yɔɔ jaa.
41006052	Baa dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ ala par ɛ, bojũu a ba ju ba wõnõ nyaar ɛ.
41006053	Ban wa gɔ̃ɔ a man do lũ a gboro a Genesaretɩ gɔ̃ɔn,
41006054	tɩ tɔ̃ɔ yi a gboro pɔ, nɩbɛ nyɛ naa a Yesu bɔ̃ɔ.
41006055	A nɩbɛ jon yɔ a wɛr 'lɔ wʋ jaa na ba tuo a ba baalsɩ nɩ sɔ̃n chiin jie jaa ban wõ ɩka wʋ be naa.
41006056	Jie jaa wʋn chen, tẽkpɛ̃ɛ pɔ bɩɩ, tẽbile pɔ bɩɩ, ka a tẽe kõkoor lɛ̃ɛɛ, ba ma gaal naa a ba baalsɩ a chãa pɔ. Ba ma sʋɔrɔ naa a Yesu ɩka wʋ sɔɔ ka ba sɩɩr a wʋ fuu nɛɛ gba, bala jaa na sɩɩr, ma sa naa.
41007001	A Faraseemɩne nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe bamɩne yi naa a Jerusalɛm wa lɔ̃ɔ a Yesu sɛ̃,
41007002	na ba nyɛ a wʋ poturbo ka ba dire nɩ nũdɛbɛ. Ka a lɛ wiil ɩka baa pɛɛ a ba nuur a, "Puorfʋ pɛɛfʋ 'lɔ ɛ."
41007003	A Faraseemɩne nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ba maa di ka bala ba pɛɛ a ba puorfʋ pɛɛfʋ 'lɔ ɛ, na ba turo a lɛ a ba nɩbɛrɛ na bin.
41007004	Bala wa yi daa wa, ba maa di ka bala ba pɛɛ a pɛɛfʋ 'lɔ ɛ. Ban turo a ba bin yɔɔ ala jũu, ba ma pɛɛn a ŋmama, dʋʋr nɩ a kulaar.
41007005	Ala lɛ so ka a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe sʋʋr a Yesu, "Bo lɛ so ka a fʋ poturbo ba turo a lɛ a sɩ nɩbɛrɛ na bin ɛ, na baa pɛɛ a ba nuur ɛ tɩ dire nɩ nũdɛbɛ!"
41007006	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ a Isaiya dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a yɩn nɛɛr ayi dẽme 'yɛr na wʋ sɛb. Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa, 'A yɩn nɩbɛ banyãna 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma naa nɩ a yɩ nɛɛ, tɩchɛ ka a yɩ pʋtɩɛr jãa a n sɛ̃.
41007007	Pɔrɔ lɛ yɩ puoro ma, bojũu yɩ wile naa nɩsaal nɛbinsɩ tɩ tɩɛr ɩka maa nɛɛ lɛ.'
41007008	Yɩ bar naa a Nãaŋmɩn Nɛɛ tɩ turo a lɛ a yɩ nɩbɛrɛ na bin.
41007009	"A ba ɩ ka yɩ de yɛ̃ bar a Nãaŋmɩn Nɛɛ tufʋ tɩ turo a lɛ a yɩn mɩ̃ɛ na bin ɛ.
41007010	Mosesɩ 'yɛr naa a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, ''Yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ sãa nɩ a fʋ ma.' Na wʋ mɩ lɛ 'yɛr, 'Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ sãa bɩɩ a wʋ ma, ba kʋ wʋ.'
41007011	Tɩchɛ ka yɩn 'yɛr ɩka a sɛɛ na, nɩrɛ wa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ sãa bɩɩ a wʋ ma, 'Bon jaa ɩn naa kʋ fʋ, n den kʋ Nãaŋmɩn.'
41007012	Yɩ maa lɛ vɛ̃ ka wʋ maal bon jaa kʋ a wʋ sãa bɩɩ a wʋ ma ɛ.
41007013	Yɩn ɩrɛ a nɩtɔ̃ jũu, ka yɩ kaara a Nãaŋmɩn Nɛɛ pɔrɔ tɩ turo a lɛ yɩn mɩ̃ɛ na bin. Yelyɔɔ mɩ ben be yɩn ɩrɛ nɩ nyɛtaa a nɩtɔ̃."
41007014	A Yesu lɛ bɔ̃ɔ bʋɔl a nɩyɔɔ ka ba lɩɛb wa a wʋ sɛ̃. Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ chɛl wõ ɩn 'yɛrɛ tɩ na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a par.
41007015	Bon jaa ba be ka a yõo ka nɩrɛ na de di ka a bʋ̃nyɩnɛ vɛ̃ ka wʋ dɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ bon 'lɔ na yi a nɩrɛ pʋtɩɛr pɔ lɛ na vɛ̃ ka wʋ dɛɛ."
41007017	Sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn wa bar a nɩyɔɔ bala tɩ kpɛ a yir, a wʋ poturbo sʋʋr wʋ naa a sʋkpa par.
41007018	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Yɩ mɩ ɩ naa a nɩbɛ bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ a par bɩɩ? Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka bon jaa ba be be ka nɩrɛ na de di na wʋ dɛɛ ɛ,
41007019	bojũu wʋ maa kpɛ a wʋ tɩɛr pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ pʋɔm lɛ wʋ ma suu na wʋ tɩ yi." Yesu 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ na wʋ wiil ɩka a bʋ̃diir a jaa sɛɛn difʋ.
41007020	Na wʋ mɩ lɛ 'yɛr ɩka, "Bon nyã na yi a nɩrɛ pʋtɩɛr pɔ lɛ ma tʋ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka wʋ dɛɛ.
41007021	Ala na ma yi a nɩrɛ pʋtɩɛr pɔ lɛ, tɩɛr dɛbɛ, nɩ a sɛ̃sɛ̃yele, nɩ a nãnyuur, nɩ nɩrɛ kʋfʋ, nɩ sɛ̃fʋ,
41007022	nɩ a nyuur, nɩ a putuo, nɩ jire, nɩ kakaba, nɩ bɔbier, nɩ yosɔ̃ɔ, nɩ pɔlyele nɩ a jɔlyele.
41007023	A yeldɛbɛ anyãna a jaa lɛ ma yi a nɩrɛ pʋtɩɛr pɔ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ dɛɛ."
41007024	Be lɛ ka a Yesu yi a be na wʋ chen a Tire wɛr pɔ. Wʋ tɩ kpɛ naa a yir ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, tɩ waa bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩrɛ jaa wʋ bɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ ben be ɛ. Tɩchɛ wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɔɔl ɛ.
41007025	Ala a pɔɔ na tara wʋ bipɔɔ ka a sɩdɛɛr tara, ajienaa wʋn wʋ wõ a Yesu 'yɛr, wʋ wan wa lo gbur dumo a wʋ niem.
41007026	A pɔɔ ba dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ ɛ, na wʋ dɔ̃ɔ yi be a Siriya Fonisiya paal pɔ. Wʋ sʋɔr naa a Yesu ɩka, wʋ dii a sɩdɛɛr bar a wʋ bipɔɔ pɔ.
41007027	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Bar ka a bibiir di a lɛ ban bʋɔrɔ, taa de a bibiir bʋ̃diir kʋ baar ɛ."
41007028	Ka a pɔɔ mɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ lɛ, n Soro, tɩchɛ a baar mɩ ma dire naa a bʋ̃ pʋr pʋr ala a bibiir na ma dire, tɩchɛ ka a loro a tẽe."
41007029	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A nɩtɔ̃ fʋn 'yɛr jũu, kulo. A sɩdɛɛr bar naa a fʋ bipɔɔ."
41007030	Wʋ kul tɩ nyɛ a bie na gã a gado ju, tɩ a sɩdɛɛr yi.
41007031	Yesu lɛ yi naa a Tire wɛr pɔ, na wʋ tu a Sidon suu a Galilee man pɔ, na wʋ tɩ chen a Dekapolisɩ paal pɔ.
41007032	Be lɛ ka nɩbɛ bamɩne waan daba na ɩ wõo, na waa tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ 'yɛrɛ sʋ̃ ɛ. Ba sʋɔr a Yesu ka wʋ sɩɩr a daba nɩ a wʋ nũu na wʋ sãa wʋ.
41007033	Ka Yesu tara a daba yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ, na wʋ de a wʋ nubie su a daba tobɔɔr pɔ, be lɛ wʋ chɩr nataar tɩ sɩɩr a daba jãlbir.
41007034	Na wʋ dʋl kaa a saaju tɩ vʋʋr na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba, "Efata!", a par lɛ a Yesu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr pɔ, yuo.
41007035	Ajienaa ka a daba tobo yuo ka a jãlbir lɩɛb ka wʋ piel 'yɛrɛ jaa chɛchɛ.
41007036	Yesu kpaal ban jũu ɩka ba taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ. Tɩchɛ a lɛ wʋn kpãa ba lɛ lɛ ba mɩ 'yɛrɛ yʋɔrɔ nɩ a jie wʋ jaa.
41007037	A nɩbɛ nɛɛ 'maan yɔɔ jaa ka ba 'yɛrɛ, "Wʋ ɩn yele jaa sʋ̃. Wʋ gba ma vɛ̃ naa ka wõo wõnõ, tɩ jãlbir lɩɛb 'yɛrɛ chɛchɛ."
41008001	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ, nɩyɔɔ lɛ lɔ̃ɔn taa go a Yesu sɛ̃, tɩ baa tara bon na di ɛ. Yesu bʋɔl a wʋ poturbo ka ba wa a wʋ sɛ̃ ka wʋ 'yɛr,
41008002	"A nɩbɛ banyã ɩrɛ naa nɩbaal, bojũu ber ata nɩ nyã ban be a n sɛ̃, baa lɛ tara bon na di ɛ.
41008003	Maa mɩ bar ba ka ba kulo nɩ a kɔ̃, ban tɩ lon sɔr pɔ, bojũu bamɩne yin tɛɛr."
41008004	Ka a wʋ poturbo 'yɛr, "Tɩchɛ nyɩnɛ lɛ a kanaa a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ nɩrɛ na nyɛ bʋ̃diir kʋ ba?"
41008005	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Paanʋ̃ɔsɩ aŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tara?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Paanʋ̃ɔsɩ ayopõi."
41008006	Wʋ 'yɛr naa a nɩbɛ, ka ba jɩ̃nɛ tẽe, tɩ na wʋ de a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ ayopõi ala puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, tɩ ŋma ŋma de kʋ a wʋ poturbo ka ba de põ a nɩbɛ.
41008007	Ba tara naa a jɩ̃bil amɩne, ka wʋ de a ala mɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, tɩ 'yɛr ɩka a poturbo ba de põ a nɩbɛ.
41008008	Ba di naa tɩɩ tɩ chɛ. Ka a wʋ poturbo wob a bʋ̃ŋmaara ala ban di faa 'yɔ̃ɔ pɛr ayopõi.
41008009	Ba ɩ naa tur anaar. Ka wʋ bar ba a sɔr.
41008010	Ajienaa, 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ poturbo 'mantaa kpɛ a gboro pɔ, na ba chen a Dalmanuta paal pɔ.
41008011	Be lɛ a Faraseemɩne wa sʋrɔ wʋ yelsʋʋrsɩ, bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bɛɛr wʋ kaa, na ba 'yɛr ɩka wʋ wiil ba jɩ̃nɛ kɔ̃ɔ ka ba bɔ̃ɔ ɩka wʋ yin a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
41008012	Ka wʋ vʋʋr lɛ fãa tɩ 'yɛr, "Bo lɛ so ka a yɩn pʋ̃pãanyã nɩbɛ bʋɔrɔ jɩ̃nɛ ɩka yɩ nyɛ? Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ jɩ̃nɛ jaa ɛ."
41008013	Wʋ bar ba naa tɩ kpɛ a gboro gɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a man gɔ̃ɔn.
41008014	A wʋ poturbo ĩin naa ba tara paanʋ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ tara bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ a gboro pɔ.
41008015	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a Faraseemɩne paanʋ̃ɔ dãbɩl nɩ a Hɛrɔd paanʋ̃ɔ dãbɩl mɩ."
41008016	Ka a wʋ poturbo guor taa 'yɛrɛ, "Sɩn ba tara a paanʋ̃ɔ lɛ so."
41008017	Yesu na bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban 'yɛrɛ, wʋ sʋʋr ba naa, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ 'yɛrɛ ɩka yaa tara paanʋ̃ɔ ɛ? Yaa bɔ̃ɔ a par sɛrɛ ɛ? A yɩ nyãa kpɛ̃mɛ na mɩ?
41008018	Yɩ tara na nɩbie tɩ ba nyɛrɛ ɛ, na yɩ tara tobo tɩ ba wõnõ ɛ. Yɩ ĩin bɩɩ?
41008019	A paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu ɩn dɔ̃ɔ de ŋma kʋ a dɔɔr tur anũu, pɛr aŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ wob a bʋ̃ŋmaar na chɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Pɛr pie nɩ ayi."
41008020	Ka a Yesu lɛ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, "Ɩn lɛ de a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ ayopõi na n ŋma kʋ a nɩbɛ tur anaar, pɛr aŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ lɛ wob 'yɔ̃ɔ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Pɛr ayopõi."
41008021	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yaa bɔ̃ɔ a par sɛrɛ ɛ?"
41008022	Ba wa ta na a Betɩsaida tẽe pɔ, ka a nɩbɛ bamɩne tara jɔ̃ɔ waan a Yesu sɛ̃ wa sʋɔr wʋ, ka wʋ sɩɩr a jɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ nyɛrɛ.
41008023	Yesu nyɔɔ naa a jɔ̃ɔ nũu tɩ tɔɔ wʋ yin a tẽe chɛchɛ. Wʋ tɩ chɩr nataar 'yɔ̃ɔ a daba nɩbie pɔ tɩ dɔɔl wʋ a nũu tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ nyɛn bon bɩɩ?"
41008024	Ka a daba dʋɔ kaa tɩ 'yɛr, "N nyɛn nɩbɛ na kaara tɩɩr kaar na ba vire yʋɔrɔ."
41008025	Ka a Yesu lɛ de a wʋ nuur pɔɔ a daba nɩbie, ka a wʋ nɩbie yuo, ka wʋ nyɛrɛ pãa nyɛ bomo a jaa chɛchɛ.
41008026	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Kulo, ta lɛ kpɛ a tẽe pɔ ɛ."
41008027	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo chen naa a tẽn ala naa gbʋr Sisariya Filipai. A sɔr pɔ ban be chiine, a Yesu sʋʋr ba naa, "An lɛ a nɩbɛ 'yɛrɛ ɩka n ɩ naa?"
41008028	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Bamɩne 'yɛr naa ɩka fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Jɔɔn 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ. Ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr ɩka Elaija. Ka a bamɩne mɩ chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ ɩka fʋ ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na dɔ̃ɔ be be."
41008029	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Tɩchɛ an lɛ yɩ mɩ 'yɛr ɩka n ɩ naa?" Ka a Pita 'yɛr, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nɩ-iraa, a Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ ɩka fʋ faa a wʋ nɩbɛ."
41008030	Ka a Yesu kpãa ba, "Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ a n 'yɛr kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ."
41008031	Yesu piel wile ba na wʋ 'yɛrɛ ɩka a Nɩsaal Bie na din dɔɔyɛ yele yɔɔ pɔ, ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ, nɩ a ba bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe tɔr wʋ bar, na ba kʋ wʋ. Tɩchɛ a ber ata daar wʋn ir naa a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋr.
41008032	Wʋ 'yɛr naa anyã chãa pɔ, ka a Pita tara wʋ yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ tɩ piel mii 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ.
41008033	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu lɩɛb kaa a wʋ poturbo tɩ mɩ mii 'yɔ̃ɔ a Pita 'yɛrɛ, "Tɔɔ chen be, Satan! A fʋ tɩɛr ɩn nɩrɛ tɩɛr, waa ɩ Nãaŋmɩn tɩɛr ɛ."
41008034	Be lɛ wʋ bʋɔl a nɩyɔɔ nɩ a poturbo ka ba wa a wʋ sɛ̃, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ turo ma, a nɩnyɩnɛ na 'laara a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩ de a daa na ɩ dɔɔyɛ nɩ kũu, tɩ turo ma.
41008035	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na bʋɔrɔ a wʋ nyɛvʋr, a wʋ nyɛvʋr na bɔr na, tɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔɔ a wʋ nyɛvʋr bɔrfʋ a maa nɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã jũu, na faa wʋ naa.
41008036	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ tara naa a wɛr nyã bonsɩ a jaa tɩ a wʋ sɩɛ wɛ, bo tɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ be be?
41008037	Bɩɩ bo lɛ nɩrɛ na de tɛɛn a wʋ sɩɛ?
41008038	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ mɩ nyɛ naa a maa nɩ a n 'yɛrbie ka a ɩ vɩ̃ yele a nɩbɛ banyã na tɔr Nãaŋmɩn bar, nɩ a putudẽme sɛ̃, a Nɩsaal Bie mɩ na kaa naa a nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ ka wʋ ɩ vĩ sʋɔ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn wa lɩɛb wa nɩ a wʋ Sãa tɩɩr 'matãan a malaka chɛchɛsɩ."
41009001	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, bamɩne ara naa a kana na ba kʋ̃ kpi ɛ, tɩchɛ na ba nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ na na wa nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ."
41009002	A ber ayʋɔb puor, Yesu tara naa Pita nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn tɛɛ na wʋ de ba nie ka ba 'mataa do tɔ̃wõo kɔ̃ɔ ju. Be lɛ wʋ tɩ chil a ba niem.
41009003	A wʋ fuu pɛl nyɩlɛ gar bʋ̃pɩla jaa nɩrɛ na maal a ka a wɛr pɔ.
41009004	Ka a Elaija nɩ a Mosesɩ, wa daa yi a ba sɛ̃. Ka bala nɩ a Yesu 'mataa 'yɛrɛ.
41009005	Ka a Pita 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Wiwile, a sɛɛ naa sɩn be a ka. Sɔɔ, ka sɩ maal sɛɛr ata: fʋ̃ʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ, Mosesɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ, Elaija mɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ."
41009006	Pita ba bɔ̃ɔ ŋmɩnɛ wʋ na 'yɛr ɛ, bojũu dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba naa.
41009007	Ka a julõjuur wa pɔɔ ba, tɩ kɔkɔr 'yɛr a be a julõjuur pɔ, "N binʋ̃nãa lɛ a nyãna. Yɩ chɛlɛ a wʋ 'yɛr."
41009008	Ajienaa ban ɩka ba kaa, baa lɛ nyɛ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ, tɩ nyɛ a Yesu tɛɛ.
41009009	Ban wa yi a tɔ̃ɔ ju suro, ka a Yesu kpãa ba ɩka ba taa wa 'yɛrɛ a lɛ ban nyɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ, wa tɩ tãn a lɛ a Nɩsaal Bie na ir yi a wʋ kũu pɔ.
41009010	Baa 'yɛr kʋ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ, tɩ 'yɛrɛ na ba sʋrɔ taa a kũu pɔ irfʋ par.
41009011	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Bo lɛ so ka a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe 'yɛr ɩka Elaija lɛ na de nie wa?"
41009012	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ a Elaija de nie wa chɔɔr a yele jaa. Tɩ ba mɩ sɛb ɩka a Nɩsaal Bie na din dɔɔyɛ yɔɔ ka ba tɔr wʋ bar.
41009013	Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a Elaija wa naa ka ba ɩ a lɛ jaa ban bʋɔrɔ kʋ wʋ nɩtãa a lɛ ban sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ."
41009014	Ban wa ta a poturbo ŋmaa bala sɛ̃, ba nyɛn nɩyɔɔ na ara jilʋ̃ ba ka a bala nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe chɩrɛ taa.
