41009015	Ka nɩbɛ na wa nyɛ a Yesu na waara, ka ba nɛɛ 'maa ka ba jo tuor puor wʋ.
41009016	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr a wʋ poturbo, "Bo lɛ yɩ chɩrɛ taa a lɛ?"
41009017	Ka nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr a be a nɩyɔɔ pɔ, "Wiwile, n bidaba lɛ sɩdɛɛr nyɔɔ ka wʋ maa tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɛ, ka n waan a fʋ sɛ̃.
41009018	'Lɔ wa ir wʋ, wʋ ma daa wʋn lɔb tẽe ka wʋ furo a natafuul tɩ ɔɔrɔ a nyɩmɛ tɩ tãa. Ka n wa sʋɔr a fʋ poturbo ɩka ba dii a sɩdɛɛr nyãna bar, ka baa tʋ̃ɔ ɛ."
41009019	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Aa, a yɩn nɩbɛ banyã na ba tara sɔɔfʋ ɛ, n be a yɩ sɛ̃ kor ta ŋmɩnɛ? N tara kãnyir ŋmɩnɛ kʋ yɩ? Waan a bie wa kʋ ma."
41009020	Ka ba waan a bie. A sɩɛ na wa nyɛ a Yesu, wʋ ir tãa a bie ka wʋ lo tẽe, mɩrɛ tɩ bile tɩ furo a natafuul.
41009021	Be lɛ a Yesu sʋʋr a bie sãa, "Sɔ̃ɔ buor lɛ a piel wʋ a nɩtɔ̃?" Ka a sãa 'yɛr, "A bibile daar jaa lɛ a piel wʋ.
41009022	Wʋ ma daa wʋn lɔb bũu pɔ bɩɩ kʋ̃ɔ pɔ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ kpi. Ala ɩ fʋn tʋ̃ɔ ɩ yele kɔ̃ɔ, kaa a sɩ nɩbaal tɩ na fʋ sʋ̃ʋ sɩ."
41009023	Ka a Yesu mɩ 'yɛr, "Bo lɛ so ka a fʋ 'yɛr ɩka ala ɩ ɩn tʋ̃ɔ naa? Yele jaa ɩn kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ kʋ a bala na sɔɔ de ma."
41009024	Ajienaa lɛ a bie sãa chɩɩr, "N sɔɔn de fʋ! Sʋ̃ʋ ma, a n sɔɔfʋ ba bɛrma ɛ!"
41009025	Yesu na wa nyɛ a nɩyɔɔ na joro lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa a jie, wʋ tãn a sɩdɛɛr, "Fʋ̃ʋ sɩdɛɛr na ma vɛ̃ ka nɩbɛ ɩ wõn, wa yi a bie pɔ na fʋ taa lɛ ɩrɛ wa kpɩɛrɛ a wʋ pɔ go ɛ!"
41009026	Ka a sɩɛ ŋme chɛlma tɩ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bie yɔɔ tɩ yi, ka a bie gã kaara fɩka kũu. Ka a nɩbɛ 'yɛr, "Wʋ kpi naa!"
41009027	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu nyɔɔ a wʋ nũu tɔɔ, ka wʋ ir ara.
41009028	Yesu na wa kpɛ a yir 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ poturbo tɛɛ, ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Bãa lɛ so ka sɩn ba tʋ̃ɔ a sɩdɛɛr nyã dii bar ɛ?"
41009029	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ tɛɛ lɛ na vɛ̃ a fʋ dii a sɩɛ nyã ka wʋ yi."
41009030	Ba yin a jie 'lɔ tɩ tu a Galilee tal. Yesu ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩrɛ jaa wʋ bɔ̃ɔ a jie ban be ɛ,
41009031	bojũu wʋ wile naa a wʋ poturbo, "Ban de naa a Nɩsaal Bie kʋ a nɩbɛ, ka ba kʋ wʋ. Ka a ber ata daar wʋn ir naa, na wʋ tara nyɛvʋr."
41009032	Tɩchɛ baa bɔ̃ɔ a par a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɩka ba sʋʋr wʋ.
41009033	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo wa ta na a Kapenahum. Ban wa kpɛ a yir, a Yesu sʋʋr ba naa, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ chɩrɛ taa a sɔr pɔ a lɛ?"
41009034	Ka ba ɩ jaa gbulo, bojũu a sɔr pɔ ba chɩrɛ na taa ɩka an lɛ ɩ a kpɛ̃ɛ.
41009035	Yesu na wa jɩ̃nɛ wʋ bʋɔl naa a wʋ poturbo Pie nɩ Ayi na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ wa bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ de nie, a nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ wʋ ɩ a yɩ jaa bile, na wʋ ɩ a yɩ jaa tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃."
41009036	Yesu vɛ̃ naa ka bibile kɔ̃ɔ ir ara a ba jaa sãlsɔɔ. Wʋ 'mɔɔn a bie tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba,
41009037	"Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na de a bibiir banyãna taaba a n jũu, maa lɛ wʋ de. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa mɩ na de ma, a ba ɩ maa lɛ wʋ de ɛ, tɩchɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma lɛ wʋ de."
41009038	Ka a Jɔɔn 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wiwile, sɩ nyɛ naa nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ na de a fʋ yuor na wʋ dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire. Ka sɩ 'yɛr ɩka wʋ bar bojũu waa ɩ a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ."
41009039	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ta dii wʋ bar ɛ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na de a n yuor tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ kʋ̃ 'yɛr ma 'yɛrdɛɛr go ɛ.
41009040	Nɩrɛ jaa na ba jɛɛr nɩ sɩ ɛ, pʋɔ sɩ naa.
41009041	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na kʋ yɩ kɔ̃'maar nɩ ŋmele, yɩn ɩ a maa sofʋ jũu, a nɩnyɩnɛ kʋ̃ wa faa a wʋ sãyar ɛ.
41009042	"Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mɩ vɛ̃ naa a bʋ̃bil banyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ na sɔɔ ma ɩ yelbier, a nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, bala 'mɔɔ nɩɛr lũ yɔɔl a wʋ nyĩe pɔ daa 'yɔ̃ɔ a man pɔ, ala sa.
41009043	Ala ɩ a fʋ nũu vɛ̃ naa ka fʋ ɩ yelbier, ŋmaa bar. Fʋn tɩ kpɛ nyɛvʋr pɔ nɩ nũŋmaa sa naa fʋn tara a nuur a jaa ayi tɩ tɩ kpɛ a wõm jie a be a bũu na ba kpĩine ɛ.
41009045	Ala ɩ a fʋ gbɛr mɩ vɛ̃ naa ka fʋ ɩ yelbier, ŋmaa bar fʋn tɩ kpɛ nyɛvʋr pɔ nɩ gbɛŋmaa sa naa fʋn tara a gbɛɛ a jaa ayi tɩ tɩ kpɛ a wõm jie.
41009047	Ala ɩ a fʋ nɩbir mɩ vɛ̃ naa ka fʋ ɩ yelbier, 'loo bar. Fʋn tɩ kpɛ Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ nɩ nɩbifɩɛ sa naa fʋn tara a nɩbie ayi tɩ tɩ kpɛ a wõm jie.
41009048	Be lɛ a 'Bufulo ba kpire ɛ, ka a bũu mɩ ba kpĩine ɛ.'
41009049	Dɔɔyɛ difʋ na lɩɛb nɩrɛ jaa nɩtãa lɛ nyaar na ma wõ bʋ̃diir ka a nʋ̃mɔ̃.
41009050	"Nyaar ɩ naa, tɩchɛ a nʋ̃ɔ wa baar, ban lɛ bʋɔl wʋn nyaar ɔ? Yɩ ɩ nyaar, na yɩ tara nyã'maar kʋ taa."
41010001	Yesu pãa yin a jie 'lɔ na wa chen a Judiya paal, na wʋ tɩ gɔ̃ɔ a Jordan man. Nɩyɔɔ lɛ wa naa a wʋ sɛ̃ go, ka wʋ wile ba nɩtãa a lɛ wʋn ma wile ba.
41010002	A Faraseemɩne bamɩne wa naa ɩka ba wa bɛɛr wʋ kaa, na ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Sɔr ben be ka daba na tɔr a wʋ pɔɔ bar bɩɩ?"
41010003	Ka a Yesu mɩ sʋʋr ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a Mosesɩ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr?"
41010004	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Mosesɩ bar sɔr ɩka daba wʋ sɛb dãasɩɛ gãn tɩ na wʋ tɔr a wʋ pɔɔ bar."
41010005	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A yɩ nyãkpɩ̃ɛn jũu lɛ so ka wʋ sɛb a lɛ.
41010006	Tɩchɛ a wɛr pielfʋ, Nãaŋmɩn maal daba nɩ pɔɔ.
41010007	A lɛ jũu, daba na bar a wʋ sãa nɩ a wʋ ma tɩchɛ ka 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ pɔɔ ɩ bʋ̃'yen,
41010008	ka ba jaa ayi ɩ ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen. Baa lɛ ɩ ayi ɛ, tɩ ɩ bʋ̃'yen.
41010009	A lɛ jũu, bon 'lɔ jaa Nãaŋmɩn na 'mataa, nɩrɛ wʋ ta nyɔɔ wɛl ɛ."
41010010	Ban wa lɩɛb kul a yir, a Yesu poturbo sʋʋr wʋ naa a 'yɛr nyã go.
41010011	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Daba jaa na tɔr wʋ pɔɔ bar tɩ kul pɔɔ yuo, wʋ maal yelbier.
41010012	Lɛ mɩ lɛ, pɔɔ wa tɔr a wʋ sɩrɛ bar tɩ kul dayuo wʋ mɩ maal yelbier."
41010013	Nɩbɛ dɔ̃ɔ waara nɩ a ba bibiir ɩka Yesu wʋ dɔɔl ba a wʋ nũu, tɩchɛ ka a wʋ poturbo mii 'yɔ̃ɔ ba.
41010014	Yesu na wa nyɛ a lɛ a wʋ poturbo na ɩ, wʋ nyɛn suur na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bar a bibiir ka ba wa a n sɛ̃, na yɩ ta ŋmaa ba sɔr ɛ. A ba nyãna taaba lɛ so a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ.
41010015	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ jaa na ba sɔɔ de a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nɩtãa a bibile ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ be ɛ."
41010016	Be lɛ wʋ 'mɔɔr a bibiir, tɩ dɔɔl ba nuur na wʋ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ ba.
41010017	Yesu na wa de a sɔr chiine, daba jon var gbur dumo a Yesu niem tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Wiwiilmɩ̃ɛ, bo lɛ ɩn maal, naa nyɛ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ?"
41010018	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ fʋ bʋɔl ma nɩmɩ̃ɛ? Nɩrɛ jaa ba ɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
41010019	Fʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa a Nãaŋmɩn Nɛɛ. Taa kʋ nɩrɛ ɛ. Taa sɛ̃nɛ ɛ. Taa juro ɛ. Taa dire dãasɩjirɩ ɛ. Taa fɔlɔ ɛ. 'Yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ sãa nɩ a fʋ ma."
41010020	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Wiwile, n bile sɔ̃ɔ jaa lɛ n turo a Nɛɛ anyãna wa tãn a dɩna."
41010021	Yesu kaa naa a daba nɩ nʋ̃fʋ, tɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A chɛ fʋn yelbʋ̃'yen. Kul tɩ da a fʋ bonsɩ a jaa de põ nɔ̃n dẽme, ala lɛ fʋn tara bʋ̃mɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃. Tɩ na fʋ pãa wa turo ma."
41010022	A 'yɛr nyã vɛ̃ naa ka a daba sɔ̃ nie na wʋ kul pʋsɔ̃ɔ, bojũu tara sʋɔ lɛ wʋ ɩ.
41010023	Be lɛ ka a Yesu kaa gʋɔr na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "A tara sʋɔ kpɛfʋ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɩn kpɛ̃ɔ!"
41010024	A 'yɛrbie anyãna vɛ̃ naa ka ba nɛɛr 'maa, tɩchɛ ka wʋ lɛ 'yɛr go, "Bibiir, a ɩn kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ nɩrɛ jaa na na kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ!
41010025	An ɩn kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃, nyɔɔma na na kpɛ kparpĩi bɔɔ pɔ gar tara sʋɔ na na kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
41010026	Ka a poturbo pãa ɩ chĩcham, tɩ lɩɛb sʋrɔ taa, "An lɛ na pãa tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ faafʋ?"
41010027	Ka a Yesu kaa ba tɩ 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ sɛ̃ 'lɔ, a ɩn tuo, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ba lɛ ɛ. Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ yele jaa ba ɩ tuo ɛ."
41010028	Be lɛ Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Nyɛ, sɩn bar bon jaa tɩ wa turo fʋ!"
41010029	Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na bar a wʋ yir bɩɩ yɛɛr, bɩɩ yɛpɔbɔ bɩɩ a wʋ sãa bɩɩ a wʋ ma, bɩɩ bibiir bɩɩ wɛr, tɩ 'la maa nɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã jũu,
41010030	wʋn nyɛn yɔɔ a dɩna. Wʋn nyɛn yie, yɛɛr, yɛpɔbɔ, mamɩne, bibiir nɩ wɛr dɔɔl gbɛɛ kɔbaa, nɩ a gefʋ! Tɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ na waara, ka wʋ nyɛ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
41010031	Tɩchɛ a nɩyɔɔ bala na de nie na wa ben puor, ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na be a puor mɩ wa de a nie."
41010032	Ba dɔ̃ɔ de a sɔr duoro a Jerusalɛm ka Yesu de a nie, tɩ a wʋ poturbo nɛɛr 'maa ka bala mɩ na turo joro dãbɩ̃ɛ. Wʋ tɔɔ naa a Pie Nɩ Ayi yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ 'yɛr kʋ ba a lɛn na wa a wʋ sɛ̃.
41010033	Yesu 'yɛr naa, "Sɩn chiine a Jerusalɛm tẽe pɔ, be lɛ ban tɩ de a Nɩsaal Bie kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe, ka ba ɩka wʋ sɛɛn kũu, na ba nyɔɔ wʋ kʋ a nɩbɛ na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ.
41010034	A banyãna na la wʋ naa, na ba chɩr nataar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, na ba fɔb wʋ tɩ kʋ wʋ. Ka a ber ata daar wʋn ir naa a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋr."
41010035	Be lɛ a Jebedee bibiir Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn tɔɔ gbʋr a Yesu na ba 'yɛr, "Wiwile, sɩ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka sɩ sʋɔr fʋ yele kɔ̃ɔ ka fʋ maal kʋ sɩ."
41010036	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Bãa lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maal kʋ yɩ?"
41010037	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Vɛ̃ ka a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jɩ̃nɛ a fʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ loor, ka 'yen mɩ jɩ̃nɛ a fʋ gʋba loor a fʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
41010038	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yaa bɔ̃ɔ a bon yɩn sʋɔrɔ ɛ. Yɩn tʋ̃ɔ nyũn a dɔɔyɛ ŋmele 'lɔ ɩn wa nyũn, bɩɩ kpɛ a dɔɔyɛ 'lɔ pɔ ɩn wa kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ kaar ɔ?"
41010039	Ka a ba 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ." Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩn nyũn a ŋmele 'lɔ ɩn na nyũn, na yɩ so a kʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn na so,
41010040	tɩchɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ loor nɩ a n gʋba loor 'lɔ n ba tara sɔr ɩka n kʋ yɩ ɛ. Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ lɛ tara sɔr ɩka wʋ de a jiir anyãna kʋ a bala wʋn chɔɔr."
41010041	A poturbo pie bala na chɛ na wa wõ a yele, ba nyɛn suur 'yɔ̃ɔ a Jemesɩ nɩ a Jɔɔn.
41010042	Ka a Yesu bʋɔl ba jaa 'mataa tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa a bala na ɩ a nãmɩne a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ma fɩrɛ naa a nɩbɛ, ka a nɩbɛrɛ ma wile a ba kpɩ̃ɛn.
41010043	A ba ɩ lɛ lɛ a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ a yɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, wʋ ɩ a yɩ jaa tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃,
41010044	ka a 'lɔ mɩ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ a nɩdiere, wʋ ɩ a yɩ jaa gbãgbaa.
41010045	A Nɩsaal Bie mɩ gba ba wa, ɩka ba wa tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ wa naa ɩka wʋ wa tʋ̃ kʋ ba, na wʋ de a wʋ nyɛvʋr lɩɛ faan nɩyɔɔ."
41010046	Ba pãa wa naa a Jeriko. Ban wa kpɛ a Jeriko tɩ yire, nɩyɔɔ turo naa Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo, ka a jɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Batimayus, Timeyus bidaba, jɩ̃nɛ a sɔr kõkoor sʋɔrɔ bomo.
41010047	Wʋn wa wõ ka a Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ lɛ, ka wʋ piel gboolo, "Yesu, David Bie, kaa n nɩbaal!"
41010048	Ka a nɩbɛ bamɩne ɩka wʋ pɔɔ a nɛɛ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ pãa chɛnɛ mal gboolo, "David Bie, kaa n nɩbaal!"
41010049	Be lɛ a Yesu tɛɛ ara tɩ 'yɛr, "Yɩ bʋɔl wʋ." Ka ba bʋɔl a jɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr wʋ, "'Maa nyãa! Ir ara, wʋ bʋɔlɔ fʋ naa."
41010050	Ka wʋ vaa ir lɔb a fɔbaa bar tɩ wa a Yesu sɛ̃.
41010051	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Bãa fʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maal kʋ fʋ?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Wiwile, n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n nyɛrɛ."
41010052	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Chiine! Fʋ sa naa, fʋn sɔɔ ma jũu." Ajienaa, wʋ nyɛrɛ naa, na wʋ turo a Yesu ka ba de a sɔr.
41011001	A lɛ ban wa gbʋrɔ a Jerusalɛm, ba ta naa a tẽn ayi, Betefagɩ nɩ Betanɩ na be a Olive tɔ̃ɔ par, ka Yesu tʋ̃ wʋ poturbo ayi.
41011002	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen a tẽbile 'lɔ na be a yɩ niem, Yɩn wa kpɩɛrɛ a tẽe pɔ, yɩn nyɛn bʋ̃bile nɩrɛ jaa na ba do wʋ sɛrɛ ɛ, ban lũ. Yɩ for waan.
41011003	Ka nɩrɛ wa sʋʋr yɩ ɩka bãa lɛ yɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ, yɩ 'yɛr wʋ ɩka, a yɩ Soro lɛ bʋɔrɔ wʋ, tɩ wʋn lɩɛb waan fɔɔ."
41011004	Ba chen tɩ nyɛ a bʋ̃bile ban lũ a yõo dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ. Ban wa foro,
41011005	nɩbɛ bamɩne na ara a be sʋʋr ba naa, "Bãa lɛ yɩ foro a bʋ̃bile ɩrɛ nɩ?"
41011006	Ka ba 'yɛr a lɛ a Yesu na ɩka ba 'yɛr, ka a nɩbɛ bar ba.
41011007	Be lɛ ba waan a bʋ̃bile wa kʋ a Yesu, na ba de a ba fɔɔr 'yɩɛr dɔɔl a bʋ̃bile ju, ka wʋ do jɩ̃nɛ.
41011008	Nɩyɔɔ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu jũu, ba den fɔɔr 'yɩɛr a sɔr pɔ, ka bamɩne mɩ kar vaɩ a por pɔ wa 'yɩɛr a sɔr pɔ.
41011009	Ka a bala na be a niem nɩ a bala na be a puor, pãa chɩlɛ gɔ̃nɔ̃ 'yɛrɛ, "Yãan yooo! Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃!
41011010	Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a sɩ sãa David nãalʋ̃ʋ na waara! Yãan yooo! Sɩ dãn Nãaŋmɩn yɔɔ jaa!"
41011011	Yesu na wa ta a Jerusalɛm, wʋ chen tɩ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ Yir kaa a bomo a jaa. A wɛr na sɔɔrɔ jũu, 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ poturbo pie nɩ ayi yin chen a Betanɩ.
41011012	A wɛr na wa chaar ka a Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo lɩɛb yi a Betanɩ waara a Jerusalɛm, kɔ̃ kpɛ naa a Yesu.
41011013	Be lɛ wʋ nyɛ a kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ tɩɛ na tɔ vaar ara a niem, ka wʋ chen ɩka wʋ tɩ kaa wɔ̃mɔ̃ ben be bɩɩ. Wʋ chen tɩ ta ka a ɩ wɔ̃mɔ̃ ba be be ɛ, vaar tɛɛ lɛ, bojũu a ba ɩ a wɔ̃mɔ̃ sɔ̃ɔ lɛ ɛ.
41011014	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a tɩɛ, "Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ lɛ wa pɔr a fʋ wɔ̃mɔ̃ di ɛ." A wʋ poturbo wõ naa a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr.
41011015	Ban wa ta a Jerusalɛm, Yesu chen tɩ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ Yir bɛchaar pɔ dire a nɩbɛ bala na chiin a bonsɩ tɩ daara nɩ a bala na daara. Wʋ daa naa libitɛɛrbɛ tɛɛbʋlsɩ lɩɛb kpa, tɩ da a bala mɩ na daara a papasɩ dakɔɔr lɔb.
41011016	Waa sɔɔ ka a nɩrɛ jaa tuo bon jaa tun a bɛchaar 'lɔ pɔ ɛ.
41011017	Be lɛ ka wʋ pãa wile ba na wʋ 'yɛr, "A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa a wʋ gãn pɔ, 'N yir ɩ naa a yir a nɩbʋrɔ ba jaa na wa puor ma,' tɩchɛ ka a yɩn 'lɔ maal wʋ a nɩfarba jie."
41011018	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃ bʋɔrɔ sɔr 'lɔ ban tu kʋ wʋ, tɩ na ba joro wʋ dãbɩ̃ɛ bojũu a nɩyɔɔ nɛɛr 'maa ba naa a wʋ wiilfʋ pɔ.
41011019	A jãanʋɔr na wa ta, Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturo lɩɛb chen a Betanɩ.
41011020	A wɛr na wa chaar bibio ka ba lɩɛb chiine a Jerusalɛm, ba nyɛ naa ka ɩ a kɔ̃kɔ̃tɩɛ na kpi lɔ̃ɔn a nyɩbɛ.
41011021	Be lɛ ka a Pita tɩɛr a lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr kʋ a tɩɛ, na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wiwile, nyɛ a tɩɛ 'lɔ fʋn pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ! Wʋ kpi naa!"
41011022	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ sɔɔ de Nãaŋmɩn.
41011023	Sɩrɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ala ɩ yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ sɔɔ naa de Nãaŋmɩn na waa baala a wʋ tɩɛr pɔ ɛ, 'lɔ gba na tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a tɔ̃ɔ nyãna, 'Ir tɩ lo a man pɔ,' a Nãaŋmɩn na sɔɔ naa ka a lɛ ɩ.
41011024	Ala lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, fʋ̃ʋ puor Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔr bon jaa tɩ sɔɔ ɩka, wʋn ɩn kʋ fʋ, wʋn ɩ naa.
41011025	Fʋ̃ʋ wa ɩka fʋ puor, tɩ tara nɩrɛ nɩ 'yɛr, vɛ̃ kʋ a nɩnyɩnɛ. A fʋ Sãa na be a saaju mɩ na vɛ̃ naa a fʋ yelbier kʋ fʋ."
41011027	Ba lɛ wa naa a Jerusalɛm go, ka a Yesu tɩ kpɛ yʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ Yir bɛchaar pɔ. A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ wa naa a wʋ sɛ̃.
41011028	Ba wa sʋʋr wʋ naa, "An lɛ kʋ fʋ a sɔr ka fʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyã? Fʋ tara naa a sɔr ɩka fʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyã ɔ?"
41011029	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N sʋʋr yɩ sʋʋrfʋ bʋ̃'yen. Yɩn wa tʋ̃ɔ wiil ma a par, n mɩ na wiil yɩ naa a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kʋ ma a sɔr ka n tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyã.
41011030	Jɔɔn na dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ wʋ a sɔr bɩɩ, nɩbɛ lɛ kʋ wʋ a sɔr? Yɩ 'yɛr n kaa!"
41011031	A ba lɩɛb chɩrɛ taa, "Sɩn be 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ tʋ̃ wʋ, wʋn sʋʋr sɩ naa, ka bo lɛ so ka saa sɔɔ wʋ ɛ?
41011032	Tɩchɛ sɩn mɩ 'yɛr ɩka nɩrɛ lɛ tʋ̃ wʋ, a ba ɩ ɛ." Ba joro naa a nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ, bojũu nɩrɛ jaa sɔɔ naa ɩka a Jɔɔn ɩn Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ.
41011033	Lɛ lɛ ba 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Saa bɔ̃ɔ ɛ." Ka a Yesu mɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N mɩ kʋ̃ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kʋ ma a sɔr ka n tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyãna ɛ."
41012001	Ka a Yesu lɛ piel 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ ba nɩ sʋkpa. Wʋ 'yɛr naa, "Daba lɛ kɔ wʋ puo na wʋ bʋr tɩwɔ̃nsɩ. Wʋ wɔɔ naa a puo wʋ jaa jilʋ̃, na wʋ tuu bɔɔ ka ban ma pɔr a wɔ̃mɔ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ na ba nɛŋmɛr ir a kʋ̃ɔ. Wʋ mɛn jie ɩ̃sʋɔ na do ka nɩrɛ na ma do jɛ̃ a be kaara a puo. Wʋ de naa a puo na wʋ kʋ nɩbɛ ɩka ba kaara tɩ na wʋ yɔ chen paal yuo pɔ.
41012002	A wɔ̃fʋ sɔ̃ɔ wa ta naa ka wʋ tʋ̃ a wʋ gbãgbaa ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩka wʋ chen a nɩbɛ bala sɛ̃ tɩ de a wɔ̃mɔ̃ amɩne.
41012003	Tɩchɛ ka ba nyɔɔ wʋ ŋme bar ka wʋ kul nũjaal.
41012004	Be lɛ wʋ lɛ tʋ̃ a gbãgbaa ɩ̃sʋɔ ka ba lɛ ŋme wʋ a ju puo tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ vĩ.
41012005	Wʋ lɛ tʋ̃n ɩ̃sʋɔ ka ba kʋ a 'lɔ. Ka wʋ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃ bamɩne, ka ba pɔb bamɩne tɩ kʋ a bamɩne.
41012006	"Wʋ chen nɩbʋ̃'yen wʋn na tʋ̃, 'lɔ lɛ a wʋ bibʋ̃'yen wʋn nʋ̃. 'Lɔ lɛ wʋ wa tʋ̃ a baaraa jaa na wʋ 'yɛr, 'Ban 'yɔ̃ɔ naa a n bie.'
41012007	"Tɩchɛ a pokaarba na wa nyɛ a bie, ba 'yɛr kʋ taa, 'A nyã lɛ ɩ a bʋ̃dire! Yɩ ɩ a sɩ kʋ wʋ, tɩ chɛ ka a bonsɩ ɩ a sɩ sofʋ.'
41012008	Be lɛ ba nyɔɔ wʋ kʋ lɔb bar a puo kõkoor.
41012009	"Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tɩɛr ɩka a puo sʋɔ na ɩ naa? Wʋn wan wa kʋ a pokaarba banyãna ba jaa tɩ de a puo kʋ nɩyor!
41012010	Yaa kar a jie nyã a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɛ? Wʋ 'yɛr ɩka, 'A kʋsɩr 'lɔ a mɩmɩɛrbɛ na tɔr bar lɛ ɩ a kʋsɩr ju.
41012011	A sɩ Soro lɛ tʋ̃ a nɩtɔ̃ ka sɔb sɩ a nɩbie.' "
41012012	Be lɛ a Juu nɩbɛrɛ bʋɔrɔ sɔr ɩka ba nyɔɔ a Yesu, bojũu ba bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka bala lɛ wʋ lɔb a sʋkpa gbɛb. Tɩchɛ ba joro naa a nɩyɔɔ bala dãbɩ̃ɛ, na ba bar wʋ tɩ lɩɛb chen.
41012013	Ba lɛ tʋ̃ naa a Faraseemɩne bamɩne nɩ nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi a nãa Hɛrɔd sɛ̃, ka ba wa bɛr Yesu nɛɛ nyɔɔ wʋ, a wʋ 'yɛrbie pɔ.
41012014	Ba wa na wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wiwile, sɩ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka fʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ. Nɩbɛ 'yɛrbie maa tʋ̃ɔ a fʋ pʋtɩɛr lɩɛb ɛ, bojũu fʋ maa chɛlɛ a lɛ nɩrɛ jaa na be ɛ. Tɩchɛ fʋ wile na a Nãaŋmɩn sɔr nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ. A tara naa sɔr ɩka sɩ yab a lõpo kʋ a nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa bɩɩ?
41012015	Sɩ yab bɩɩ sɩ ta yab ɛ?" Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu bɔ̃ɔn a ba nɛbɛr yele ban waan, na wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Bo lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ bɛɛr ma kaa? Yɩ de a libir ɩ̃sʋɔ waan ka n kaa."
41012016	Be lɛ ba de a libir kur ɩ̃sʋɔ waan, ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "An foto nɩ a yuor lɛ be a libir pɔ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Siisa lɛ."
41012017	Lɛ lɛ ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ de a 'lɔ na ɩ a Siisa sofʋ na yɩ yab wʋ, na yɩ mɩ de a 'lɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sofʋ na yɩ mɩ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn." Ka ba faa tɩ nyɔɔr a nɛɛr ara nɩ.
41012018	A nɩbɛ bamɩne ban bʋɔlɔ a Saduseemɩne na 'yɛr ɩka kũu pɔ irfʋ ba be be ɛ, mɩ wa naa wa sʋʋr wʋ,
41012019	"Wiwile, Mosesɩ sɛb kʋ sɩ ɩka nɩrɛ yɛbɛ wa kpi tɩ bar pɔɔ na ba tara bie ɛ, a wʋ yɛbɛ wʋ kul a pɔɔkʋɔr 'lɔ na wʋ dɔɔ bibiir kʋ a wʋ yɛbɛ 'lɔ na kpi.
41012020	Yɛɛr ayopõi lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be, ka ba kpɛ̃ɛ kul pɔɔ kpi tɩ chɛ bar, waa tara bie ɛ.
41012021	Ka a wʋ turo de a pɔɔkʋɔr kul, baa mɩ dɔɔ bie ɛ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ mɩ kpi. A lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a turo ata sʋɔ.
41012022	Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa a yɛɛr ayopõi banyãna ba jaa kulnaa a pɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, tɩ waa dɔɔ bie ɛ, a baaraa jaa ka a pɔɔ mɩ kpi.
41012023	Bala wa ir yi a kũu pɔ, an pɔɔ lɛ wʋn ɩ, an ɩ ba jaa kul wʋn lʋɔr taa?"
41012024	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yaa nyɛ yɩn bɔr, bojũu yaa bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛbɛ nɩ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ ɛ.
41012025	Nɩbɛ wa ir a kũu pɔ ba kʋ̃ lɛ kul taa ɛ, tɩ ban kaara naa fɩka a malakasɩ, baa kulo taa ɛ.
41012026	A kũu pɔ irfʋ yele yɩ kar a Mosesɩ gãn pɔ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn nyɛ a tɩbile na 'lɩrɛ bũu, ka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'N ɩ naa a Abraham Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Isaakɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Jekɔb Nãaŋmɩn.'
41012027	Wʋ ɩ naa vʋr Nãaŋmɩn, waa ɩ kũn Nãaŋmɩn ɛ. Yɩ tul naa."
41012028	A Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wile ɩ̃sʋɔ wa ara na chɛl a lɛ a Yesu nɩ a nɩbɛ na 'mataa 'yɛrɛ. Ka wʋ nyɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr nʋ̃mɔ̃. Ka wʋ mɩ sʋʋr a Yesu, "A Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛr a jaa pɔ, buor sʋɔ lɛ ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ?"
41012029	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A 'lɔ na ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar a jaa nɩ nyã, 'A Isɩral nɩbɛ, yɩ chɛlɛ! A sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn, wʋ ɩ naa Soro bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ.
41012030	Nʋ̃ a fʋ Soro Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a fʋ nyãa, nɩ a fʋ nyɛvʋr wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ tɩɛr wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ kpɛ̃ɔ wʋ jaa.'
41012031	A 'lɔ na tu nɩ nyã, 'Nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ nɩtãa lɛ fʋn nʋ̃ a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ.' Nɛɛ jaa ba be be ɩ kpɛ gar a anyã ɛ."
41012032	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "Wiwile, fʋ 'yɛr yelmɩ̃ɛ, a lɛ fʋn 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ be be, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba lɛ be be pʋɔ wʋ ɛ.
41012033	A fʋ nʋ̃ wʋ nɩ a fʋ nyãa, nɩ a fʋ tɩɛr wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ kpɛ̃ɔ wʋ jaa, na fʋ lɛ nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ nɩtãa a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ, a yele anyãna tufʋ ɩn gar dʋ̃n fʋn kʋ chʋm kʋ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ bɔɔrlorsɩ a jaa."
41012034	Yesu na nyɛ a lɛ a daba na 'yɛr nɩ yɛ̃ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Faa jãa nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ ɛ." An yi a be chiine nɩrɛ jaa ba lɛ 'la sʋʋr wʋ sʋʋrfʋ go ɛ.
41012035	A lɛ a Yesu na wile a Puorfʋ Yir bɛchaar pɔ, wʋ sʋʋr naa a nɩbɛ, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a ta ka a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe 'yɛr ɩka David bie lɛ a Nɩ-iraa?
41012036	A ba ɩ a David mɩ̃ɛ pɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ, ka wʋ 'yɛr ɩka, 'A n Soro Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ a n Soro nyã wʋn ir, "Jɩ̃nɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ loor ka n wa de a fʋ dɔ̃dẽme bin a fʋ gbɛɛ pĩlem." '
41012037	Ala ɩ David mɩ̃ɛ bʋɔl wʋ naa a wʋ Soro, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ wʋn lɛ ɩ a wʋ bie tɛɛ?" Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala ara chɛlɛ wʋ nɩ pʋpɛl.
41012038	Yesu wile naa tɩ na wʋ kpãa ba, "Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe sɛ̃, ba ma su naa a fuu vɛɛsɩ ala yʋɔrɔ ɩka ba puor ba a dar pɔ.
41012039	Bala be wa kpɛ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie, a niem lɛ ba ma jɩ̃nɛ.
41012040	Ba mɩ ma fɔlɔ naa a pɔɔkɔɛ, na ba mɩ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn kor, bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩbɛ ba kaara ba. A nɩbɛ banyãna 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ na kpɛ̃mɛ naa."
41012041	Yesu jɛ̃n gbʋr a jie ban 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a libie a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ Yir pɔ, na wa kaara a lɛ a nɩyɔɔ na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a ba libie. Taraa dẽme yɔɔ jaa lɔɔrɔ naa yɔɔ.
41012042	Be lɛ ka a pɔɔkɔnɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ mɩ be be na wʋ mɩ waan libikue ayi na ɩ kobo wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a libie pɔ.
41012043	Ka Yesu bʋɔl a wʋ poturbo ka ba tɔɔ gbʋr wʋ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a pɔɔkɔnɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ nyã lɔb gar ba jaa.
41012044	A tara dẽme ma 'yɔ̃ɔn tɩ chɛ a libiyɔɔ amɩne, tɩchɛ a pɔɔkɔnɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ nyã 'lɔ, a jaa lɛ wʋ de 'yɔ̃ɔ. Waa lɛ tara bon jaa go ɛ."
41013001	Yesu na wa yire a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ Yir pɔ, a wʋ poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wiwile, nyɛ a kʋsɩbɛ ban mɛn a yir kpɛ̃ɛ nyã ka wʋ kaara ka!"
41013002	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr sɔɔ wʋ, "Mɩ fʋ nyɛ naa a lɛ ban mɛ a yir kpɛ̃ɛ nyãna? A kʋsɩvɩɛl anyãna 'yen jaa kʋ̃ lɛ wa chɛnɛ dɔɔl wʋ tɔ ju ɛ. Ban dãn a jaa lɔb."
41013003	Yesu na wa jɩ̃nɛ a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ ju, a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ Yir nidaa, Pita nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn nɩ Andiru sʋʋr wʋ naa a ba tɛɛ,
41013004	"'Yɛr kʋ sɩ a daar 'lɔ a anyã na ɩ. Bo lɛ na ɩ a jɩ̃nɛ sɛrɛ tɩ chɛ ka a wa ɩ?"
41013005	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ka nɩrɛ jaa ta wa bɛl yɩ ɛ!
41013006	Nɩyɔɔ na de naa maa yuor waan wa 'yɛrɛ, 'Maa lɛ a Yesu,' na ba wa bɛlɛ nɩyɔɔ.
41013007	Yɩn wa wõn tam, ka ba 'yɛrɛ a tam 'yɛr, yɩ taa mɩrɛ ɛ. A lɛ na ɩ naa, tɩchɛ a wɛr baarfʋ chɛnɛ na be puor.
41013008	Nɩbʋr dẽdẽme na yin tam, ka a nãmɩne mɩ yi tam. Ka a tẽgãn dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ jiir yɔɔ, ka kɔ̃ mɩ lo. A dɔɔyɛ anyãna lɛ ɩ a pielfʋ.
41013009	"Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn, ɩka ban ma nyɔɔr yɩn chiin a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie, na ba lɛ pɔb yɩ, a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir. A maa yɩn sɔɔ jũu, ban tara yɩn chiin a tẽe nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nãmɩne jie, ɩka ba tɩ tɔɔr a yɩ 'yɛr, tɩ yɩn tu naa a be 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ ba.
41013010	A 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã na den nie ta a nɩbʋrɔ ba jaa.
41013011	Bala wa nyɔɔr yɩ chiin a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka tɩɛr nyɔɔ yɩ a lɛ yɩn tɩ 'yɛr ɛ. Lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn na wiil yɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ sɔ̃ɔ, 'yɛr wʋ. A ba ɩ yɩn lɛ 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ a 'yɛrbie yi naa a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛ̃.
41013012	"Yɛbɛ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ yɛbɛ, ka ba kʋ wʋ, ka a sãa mɩ gar 'yɔ̃ɔ bie, ka ba kʋ wʋ. Bibiir kʋ̃ lɛ wõnõ a ba sãamɩne toor ɛ, na ba vɛ̃ ka ba kʋ a ba sãamɩne.
41013013	Nɩrɛ jaa na 'laar yɩ naa, yɩn sɔɔ ma jũu, tɩ 'lɔ na sɔɔ tɩ ta a baaraa, na nyɛn Nãaŋmɩn faafʋ.
41013014	"Yɩn nyɛ naa a yele 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na 'laar na be a jie 'lɔ an ba sɛɛ ɛ, na wʋ sɔ̃ɔ a jie, na wʋ vɛ̃ ka a wʋ suur dire. A fʋ̃ʋ nyã na kara bɔ̃ɔ a par. Yɩn wa nyɛ a lɛ, nɩbɛ na be a Judiya ba jo do a tɔ̃ɔ ju.
41013015	Nɩrɛ jaa na be gar ju, ta suu a die pɔ tɩ de bon jaa ɛ.
41013016	'Lɔ mɩ na be a puo pɔ, ta lɛ chen tɩ de a wʋ fɔbaa ɛ.
41013017	A bɩbir nyãna an ɩn tuo kʋ a pɔɔpʋʋr nɩ a bala na tara a bi'yɛnsɩ.
41013018	Yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka a ta wa ɩ uon ɛ.
41013019	A ber ala pɔ, nɩbɛ na din dɔɔyɛ yɔɔ. Nãaŋmɩn na maal a wɛr baa di a dɔɔyɛ nyã bʋrɔ ɛ, tɩ ba mɩ kʋ̃ lɛ wa di wʋ go ɛ.
41013020	Ala ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn ba ŋmaa a ber ala bar ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ chɛ ɛ. Tɩchɛ a bala wʋn chɛl ir jũu, wʋ ŋmaan bar.
41013021	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, nɩrɛ wa 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka yɩ nyɛ a Nɩ-iraa a ka, bɩɩ kasɛn lɛ wʋ be, yɩ taa sɔɔrɔ ɛ.
41013022	Bojũu a jire Nɩ-iraa nɩ a jire 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na wa na wa tʋ̃nɔ̃ a lɛ a nɩbɛ na ba dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ ɛ, na ba maala yelbɛrɛ fɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ ba a kpɛ̃ɔ. Na ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bɛl a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na chɛl ir, ala ɩ ban tʋ̃ɔ naa.
41013023	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn! N den nie 'yɛr kʋ yɩ.
41013024	"Tɩchɛ a dɔɔyɛ nyã baarfʋ sɔ̃ɔ, 'Mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na lii naa, ka a ŋmɛraa kʋ̃ mɩ lɛ chaar ɛ,
41013025	Ka a ŋmɛrbie pɔrɔ yire a saaju loro, tɩ a saaju wʋ jaa dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.'
41013026	"A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, ban nyɛn a Nɩsaal Bie na waara a julõjuur pɔ, nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ tɩɩr.
41013027	Wʋn tʋ̃ naa a wʋ malakasɩ, ka ba wa lɔ̃ɔ taa a bala wʋn chɛl ir a wɛr wʋ jaa, tɩ yin a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie tɩ tɔ a mʋrfʋ jie.
41013028	"Yɩ de a pɔlpɔl tɩɛ yele jãn yɛ̃. 'Lɔ wa tʋɔrɔ a vaar yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a tʋl sɔ̃ɔ gbʋr naa.
41013029	A lɛ mɩ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ, yɩn wa nyɛ a lɛ n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ na ɩrɛ, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a sɔ̃ɔ gbʋr naa jaa yɛ̃yɛ̃.
41013030	N 'yɛrɛ naa yelmɩ̃ɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ɩka a pʋ̃pãanyã nɩbɛ kʋ̃ kpi baar ɛ, tɩ yɩ nyɛ a yele anyãna ka a ɩ.
41013031	A saaju nɩ a wɛr na wa baar naa tɩchɛ maa 'yɛrbie dɔ̃ɔ kʋ̃ wa baar ɛ.
41013032	"Nɩrɛ jaa ba bɔ̃ɔ a bɩbir nyã ɛ, bɩɩ a sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a malakasɩ gba na be a saaju ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a Bie mɩ ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a Sãa tɛɛ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ.
41013033	Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ vɩla! Yɩ kaar sʋ̃! Yaa bɔ̃ɔ a sɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
41013034	An kaar naa fɩka yir sʋɔ na wa yʋɔrɔ tɩ de a wʋ yir 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ nuur pɔ, na wʋ kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa nɩ wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃, tɩ mɩ 'yɛr kʋ a dɔ̃dɔr guro ka wʋ kaara.
41013035	A lɛ jũu yɩ kaara tɩ guro wʋ, bojũu yaa bɔ̃ɔ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a yir sʋɔ na na lɩɛb wa ɛ. Amɩne kɔ̃ɔ a wa ɩ jãanʋɔr, bɩɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ bɩ̃ɩn, bɩɩ nɔrsɩ na kõnõ, bɩɩ bibio pipi.
41013036	Yɩ ta wa vɛ̃ ka wʋ wa dũu yɩ a yɩ be gʋ̃ɔ pɔ ɛ.
41013037	A lɛ n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ, nɩrɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ kaar sʋ̃!"
41014001	A chen ber ayi ka ban di a Gõl Bar Difʋ nɩ a Paanʋ̃kõo Lɔ̃ɔfʋ, ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe bʋɔrɔ vuo 'lɔ ban na tu sɔɔl nyɔɔ a Yesu kʋ.
41014002	Tɩchɛ ka ba 'yɛr, "A ta ɩ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, ka a jɛɛr taa ir a chara pɔ ɛ."
41014003	Yesu na wa be a Betanɩ a Simon 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a kɔ̃kɔn yir, ka ba 'mataa dire, pɔɔ kɔ̃ɔ wa waan na pɩ̃rtɔvɩla nɩ kãnyũu kɔ̃ɔ dafʋ na ba wõnõ ɛ. A pɔɔ kpɩr naa a pɩ̃rtʋɔ nyĩe tɩ kpaar a kãnyũu ala dɔɔl a Yesu ju.
41014004	Ka a nɩbɛ bala na be be nyɛ suur tɩ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Bo lɛ so ka wʋ sɔ̃ɔ a kãnyũu nyã bar a nɩtɔ̃?
41014005	Wʋn taa den da nɩbʋ̃'yen yuon gbul sãyar libie na wʋ de kʋ nɔ̃n dẽme." Tɩ mii 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɔɔ.
41014006	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bar wʋ! Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ mii 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ? Wʋ maal vɩla kʋ ma.
41014007	A nɔ̃n dẽme 'lɔ, yɩn nɩ bala ben ka. Yɩn tʋ̃ɔ sʋ̃ʋ ba sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa yɩn bʋɔrɔ, tɩchɛ maa kʋ̃ be a yɩ sɛ̃ sɔ̃ɔ jaa ɛ.
41014008	Wʋ ɩ naa a lɛ wʋn tʋ̃ɔ. Wʋ kpaar a kãnyũu 'yɔ̃ɔ ma tɩ chɛ ka n ba kpi sɛrɛ ɛ, na wʋ chɔɔr ma guro nɩ a n ũufʋ.
41014009	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, jie jaa ban wa 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna a wɛr wʋ jaa pɔ, ban 'yɛr naa a lɛ a pɔɔ nyã na ɩ na ba chɛnɛ tara a wʋ tɩɛr."
41014010	A Pie nɩ Ayi bala wʋn kaa ir ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Judas Isɩkariyot chen a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr ba ɩka wʋ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka wʋ de a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba nuur pɔ.
41014011	Ban wa wõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr ka a nʋ̃mɔ̃ ba, ka ba 'yɛr ɩka ban kʋ wʋn libie. Ka a Judas pãa bʋɔrɔ vuo 'lɔ wʋn na tu de a Yesu kʋ ba.
41014012	A bɩbir dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩ naa a Paanʋ̃kõo Lɔ̃ɔfʋ, ka ban na kʋ a pele na ba di a Gõl Bar Difʋ, Yesu poturbo sʋʋr wʋ naa, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ chen tɩ chɔɔr a Gõl Bar nyã bʋ̃diir a fʋ tɩ di?"
41014013	Wʋ tʋ̃ naa a wʋ poturbo ayi, na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen a tẽe pɔ, daba na tuo kʋ̃ɔ nɩ dʋʋ na tuor yɩ naa. Yɩ turo wʋ.
41014014	A yir 'lɔ pɔ wʋn wa tɩ kpɛ, yɩ sʋʋr a yir sʋɔ, 'A Wiwile ɩka sɩ wa sʋʋr fʋ, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ a 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ poturbo na wa 'mataa di a Gõl Bar Difʋ?" '
41014015	Wʋn wiil yɩ naa bɔɔpɩɛ ban chɔɔr. Yɩ maal a bʋ̃diir a be."
41014016	Ba yin chen a tẽe tɩ nyɛ a lɛ jaa a Yesu na 'yɛr kʋ ba. Ka ba maal a Gõl Bar bʋ̃diir.
41014017	Jãanʋɔr na wa ta, Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo Pie nɩ Ayi wa naa.
41014018	Ban wa dire, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na tɩ gar 'yɔ̃ɔ ma; ɩ̃sʋɔ sɩn 'mataa dire nɩ a labʋ̃'yen pɔ."
41014019	Be lɛ ka ba jaa pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ ka ba sʋrɔ wa bʋ̃'yen 'yen, "Maa lɛ ɔ?"
41014020	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "A yɩ Pie nɩ Ayi ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ! A yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ sɩn 'mataa tũno a labʋ̃'yen pɔ lɛ.
41014021	A Nɩsaal Bie na kpi naa nɩtãa lɛ ban sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ. Tɩchɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nɩsaal Bie na din dɔɔyɛ gar nɩrɛ jaa! Ka bala ta ba dɔɔ wʋ ɛ, ala sa."
41014022	Ban wa dire ka a Yesu de a paanʋ̃ɔ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, tɩ ŋmaa de kʋ a wʋ poturbo, na wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ de, a n ɩ̃gãn lɛ."
41014023	Wʋ lɛ den a ŋmele 'lɔ ban nyuro nɩ, na wʋ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan tɩ lɛ de kʋ ba, ka ba jaa nyũ.
41014024	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N jɩ̃ɩ lɛ a anyã na vɛ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛtɩraa na tara kpɛ̃ɔ, an chir naa, na a faa nɩyɔɔ.
41014025	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, n kʋ̃ lɛ nyũ a dãa anyãna ɛ, wa tɩ tãn a daar 'lɔ ɩn na nyũ a bʋ̃paalaa a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
41014026	Ban wa yiel yiel dãn Nãaŋmɩn, ba suun chen a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ ju.
41014027	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ jaa na jon tɩ bar ma, nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛr a wʋ gãn pɔ, Ɩn ŋme naa pɛchinɛ kʋ ka a piir yɛ̃yɛl.
41014028	Tɩchɛ maa wa ir a kũu pɔ, ɩn de yɩn nie chen a Galilee."
41014029	Ka a Pita chɛ nyãa 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ gba, ba jaa sɔɔn bar fʋ tɩ maa 'lɔ kʋ̃ bar fʋ ɛ."
41014030	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a Pita, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, dɩna tɩ̃sɔɔ, a nɔrdɔ̃ɔ kʋ̃ kõ gbɛɛ ayi sɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ fʋ 'yɛr gbɛɛ ata ɩka faa bɔ̃ɔ ma ɛ."
41014031	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita 'yɛr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa ɩka, "Maa nɩ fʋ̃ʋ na 'mantaa kpi gba, tɩ n kʋ̃ 'yɛr ɩka n ba bɔ̃ɔ fʋ ɛ." Ka a bala mɩ na chɛ 'yɛr a lɛ nɛ.
41014032	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo chen naa a jie 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Getɩsemanɩ, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ jɩ̃nɛ a kana, tɩ ka n chen tɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn."
41014033	Be lɛ wʋ tara Pita nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn 'mataa chiin ka a wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ jaa, ka tɩɛr nyɔɔ wʋ yɔɔ.
41014034	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N tɩɛr sɔ̃ɔ naa, tɩ nyɛtãan kũu. Yɩ jɩ̃nɛ a kana gu ma tɩ na yɩ taa guro ɛ."
41014035	Wʋ chen naa a niem bɩ̃lãa tɩ lo kpa tẽe sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɩka ala ɩ a tara naa ɩfʋ kɔ̃ɔ, wʋ vɛ̃ ka a sɔ̃ɔ nyãna po wʋ.
41014036	Wʋ 'yɛr naa, "N Sãa, yele jaa ba gar a fʋ maalfʋ ɛ. De a dɔɔyɛ ŋmele nyãna bar a n sɛ̃, tɩchɛ a ta tu maa bɔfʋ ɛ, a tu a lɛ fʋ̃ʋ na bʋɔrɔ."
41014037	Wʋ lɩɛb chen a poturbo sɛ̃ tɩ nyɛ ka a ɩ ba gur naa. Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Simon Pita, "Simon, fʋ guro naa ɔ? A fʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ jɛ̃ bɩ̃lãa gu ma ɛ?
41014038	Yɩ jɛ̃ gu chɛlɛ, na yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka a bɛɛrkaa ta wa tʋ̃ɔ yɩ ɛ. A yɩ tɩɛr 'lɔ bʋɔrɔ naa tɩchɛ ka a yɩ ɩ̃gãma ba tʋɔr ɛ."
41014039	Wʋ lɛ chen naa tɩ puor a Nãaŋmɩn a lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju.
41014040	Wʋ lɩɛb wa nyɛ ba go ka a ɩ ba gur naa bojũu gʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ba naa. Baa bɔ̃ɔ ŋmɩnɛ ban lɛ 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu ɛ.
41014041	Wʋ lɩɛb wa a ba sɛ̃ a gbɛɛ ata sɔ̃ɔ wa sʋʋr ba, "Yɩ chɛnɛ na gã guro na yɩ pɛ̃nɛ ɔ? A sɛɛ naa! A sɔ̃ɔ ta naa. Nyɛ, ba gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nɩsaal Bie kʋ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ!
41014042	Yɩ vaa ir, ka sɩ chen a ba sɛ̃. Nyɛ, a n gagaraa na waara!"
41014043	Yesu na chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ lɛ ka Judas na ɩ a wʋ poturo pie nɩ ayi ɩ̃sʋɔ tɩ daasãa, nɩ nɩbɛ na tara sɔbɛrɛ nɩ dakʋrsɩ waara nɩ a Yesu nyɔɔfʋ jie. A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ lɛ tʋ̃ ba.
41014044	Judas dɔ̃ɔ wiil a nɩbɛ mana ɩka, "A 'lɔ ɩn na tɩ puor mʋʋr a kɔtɩr yɩ nyɔɔ a 'lɔ, na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ tara wʋ chiin."
41014045	Ban wa ta, Judas pɔɔn chen a Yesu sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "Wiwile!" Tɩ puor wʋ nɩ mʋʋrfʋ.
41014046	Ka a bala wʋn chiin nyɔɔ a Yesu.
41014047	Be lɛ ka a bala ɩ̃sʋɔ na ara gbʋr a Yesu vʋ̃ɔ a wʋ sʋɔ chɛn a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãa gbãgbaa toor ŋmaa.
41014048	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "A mɔ̃ nɩbier lɛ n ɩ ka yɩ waan sɔbɛrɛ, nɩ dakʋrsɩ a n nyɔɔfʋ jie ɔ?
41014049	Bɩbir jaa lɛ n ma dɔ̃ɔ be a yɩ sɛ̃, na n wile yɩ a Puorfʋ Yir pɔ, tɩ yaa nyɔɔ ma ɛ. Tɩchɛ a ɩ naa a lɛ ɩka a tu a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr."
41014050	Be lɛ a Yesu poturbo ba jaa bar wʋ tɩ jo.
41014051	Pɔlbile kɔ̃ɔ mɩ na vaar fɔbaa tɛɛ turo nɩ a Yesu, ba nyɔɔ wʋ naa.
41014052	Ka wʋ mɩɩr a fɔbaa 'yɔ̃ɔ ba tɩ jon sal'mʋɔr.
41014053	Be lɛ ba chiin a Yesu a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãa yir, ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ ba jaa nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ 'matãan a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe, na ɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ nɩbɛrɛ, wa lɔ̃ɔ taa.
41014054	Pita mɩ turo naa a puor jaa na wʋ wa tɩ kpɛ a bɔɔrlo nãa yir bɛchaar pɔ, na wʋ 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a bala na kara a Puorfʋ Yir uoro bũu.
41014055	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ nɩbɛrɛ na chɛ bʋɔrɔ yele kɔ̃ɔ na wiil ɩka Yesu sɛɛn kũu, tɩ baa nyɛ ɛ.
41014056	Nɩyɔɔ mɩ ŋman jirsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, tɩchɛ a ba 'yɛrbie ŋma taa poe.
41014057	Ka a bamɩne mɩ ir ŋmaa jire 'yɛr ɩka,
41014058	"A ba sɛ̃, wʋ 'yɛr naa ɩka, 'A Puorfʋ Yir nyãna a nɩrɛ nũu na mɛ, ɩn ŋmɛr wʋ naa tɩ na n de ber ata mɛn 'lɔ na ba ɩ nɩrɛ nũu bʋ̃mɩɛraa ɛ.' "
41014059	Tɩchɛ a ba 'yɛr mɩ ba ɩ bʋ̃'yen ɛ.
41014060	Be lɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãa ir ara tɩ sʋʋr a Yesu, "Faa 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr sɔɔrɔ ba bɩɩ? Bo dãasɩɛsɩ lɛ anyãna ban dire dɔɔlɔ fʋ. A ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ ɔ?"
41014061	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu ɩ jaa gbul, waa 'yɛr sɔɔ wʋ ɛ. Ka a bɔɔrlo nãa lɛ sʋʋr wʋ go, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ sɩn 'Yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Bie na ɩ a Nɩ-iraa ɔ?"
41014062	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ. Yɩn nyɛ naa a Nɩsaal Bie na jɩ̃nɛ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ nũsʋ̃ɔ loor. Yɩ mɩ na lɛ nyɛn wʋn waara a julõjuur pɔ."
41014063	Ka a bɔɔrlo nãa tɔɔ a fuu chɩɛr nɩ suur, tɩ sʋʋr, "Bãa lɛ sɩn lɛ bʋɔrɔ nɩrɛ ɩka wʋ lɛ 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr go?
41014064	Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ wõ naa a lɛ wʋn fere. Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ tɩɛr?" Ka ba jaa 'yɛr ɩka wʋ sɛɛn kũu.
41014065	Be lɛ a bamɩne piel chɩrɛ nataar 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ, ka a bamɩne mɩ pɔɔ a wʋ nɩbie tɩ ŋme wʋ, tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Wiil sɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ŋme fʋ." Ka a bala mɩ na guro a Puorfʋ Yir mɩ ŋme ŋme wʋ.
41014066	Pita jɩ̃nɛ naa a be a bɛchaar pɔ, ka a bɔɔrlo nãa gbãgbapɔɔbile ɩ̃sʋɔ wa wa.
41014067	Wʋn wa nyɛ a Pita na uoro a bũu, wʋ kaa wʋ naa lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ 'yɛr, "Fʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ turo a Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ."
41014068	Ka a Pita chɩɩr tɩ 'yɛr, "N ba bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ fʋn 'yɛrɛ par ɛ." Tɩ na wʋ tɔɔ chen tɩ ara a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ.
41014069	A pɔɔbile na wa nyɛ a Pita a be, wʋ lɛ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ na ara a be, "A nyã mɩ ɩ naa a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ."
41014070	Ka a Pita lɛ chɩɩr go. A ba kor ɛ, tɩ a bala na ara gbʋr a Pita mɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, fʋ ɩ naa a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ, bojũu Galilee lɛ fʋ mɩ yi."
41014071	Ka a Pita pɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, tɩ pɔrɔ kʋrɔ ba 'yɛrɛ ɩka, "N ba bɔ̃ɔ a daba nyã 'yɛr yɩn 'yɛr ɛ."
41014072	Ajienaa lɛ ka a nɔraa mɩ tɔ̃ɔ kõ a gbɛɛ ayi sʋɔ. Ka a Pita pãa tɩɛrtɔ a lɛ a Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Fʋn chɩɩr ma naa gbɛɛ ata, tɩ ka a nɔrdɔ̃ɔ kõ gbɛɛ ayi." Pita na wa tɩɛr bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ, ka wʋ kõ yɔɔ jaa.
41015001	A wɛr na wa chaar bibio, a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ ba jaa nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ nɩbɛrɛ na chɛ, lɔ̃ɔn guor taa lũ a Yesu tara wʋ chiin tɩ kʋ a nãa Pilate.
41015002	Ka a Pilate sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa ɔ?" Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, a ɩn a lɛ fʋn 'yɛr."
41015003	Ka a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Yesu yuor.
41015004	Be lɛ a Pilate sʋʋr a Yesu, "Faa 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr jaa ɛ, nyɛ lɛ ban sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ fʋ a yuor jɩ̃!"
41015005	Tɩchɛ Yesu ba haa nɛɛ ɛ, ka a 'maa a Pilate nɛɛ.
41015006	A mɩ ɩ naa a ba tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ ka bala wa lɔ̃ɔ taa dire a Gõl Bar Difʋ, a ba nãa ma ir nɩrɛ 'lɔ a nɩbɛ na bʋɔrɔ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ bar.
41015007	Barabasɩ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ pʋɔ a nɩbɛ bamɩne pɔ, na dɔ̃ɔ ir jɛɛr nɩ a paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na ba kʋ nɩbɛ, ka ba nyɔɔr ba pɔɔ.
41015008	Nɩyɔɔ wa naa a Pilate sɛ̃ wa sʋɔr wʋ ɩka, wʋ ɩ kʋ ba a lɛ wʋn ma ɩ.
41015009	Ka a Pilate sʋʋr ba, "Yɩ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n ir a Juu nɩbɛ nãa kʋ yɩ bɩɩ?"
41015010	Pilate bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a nyuur ban tara nɩ a Yesu lɛ vɛ̃ ban nyɔɔ wʋ waan a wʋ sɛ̃.
41015011	Tɩchɛ ka a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ dʋ̃ a nɩbɛ toor ɩka, ba 'yɛr ɩka, wʋ yuo a Barabasɩ bar.
41015012	Ka a Pilate sʋʋr ba go, "Tɩ n ɩ ŋmɩnɛ nɩ a 'lɔ yɩn bʋɔlɔ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa?"
41015013	Ka ba tãn, "Kpa wʋ a daa ju!"
41015014	Be lɛ ka a Pilate sʋʋr ba, "Bãa wʋ ɩ? Bo tʋ̃dɛɛr lɛ wʋ tʋ̃?" Tɩchɛ ka ba tãna kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, "Kpa wʋ a daa ju!"
41015015	Pilate na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ pɛl a nɩbɛ pʋɔ jũu, wʋ yuo naa a Barabasɩ kʋ ba. Wʋ vɛ̃ naa ka ba fɔb a Yesu yɔɔ jaa, tɩ de wʋ kʋ a sojasɩ ɩka, ba tɩ kpa wʋ a daa ju, ka wʋ kpi.
41015016	Be lɛ a sojasɩ tara a Yesu kpɛ̃n a nãa yir kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ pɔ, tɩ bʋɔl a ba taaba sojasɩ lɔ̃ɔ taa.
41015017	Ba den fuu jɩɛ nãa fuu kaar su wʋ, na ba lɛ de gʋʋr vil nãa jupil kaar su wʋ.
41015018	Tɩ pãa piel laara wʋ, "Yãan yooo, Juu nɩbɛ nãa!"
41015019	Tɩ ma de daa ŋmen wʋ a jũu tɩ chɩrɛ nataar 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ. Ba gbur dumo a wʋ niem puoro wʋ.
41015020	Ban wa la wʋ a nɩtɔ̃ wa baar, ba yaa naa a fuu 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ bar, tɩ de a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ fuu su wʋ, na ba pãa de wʋ chiin ɩka ba tɩ kpa wʋ a daa ju.
41015021	A sɔr pɔ, ba nyɛn Simon na yi Sirenɩ tẽe pɔ, Aleksanda nɩ Worofʋs sãa lɛ. Mʋɔ pɔ lɛ wʋ yi tala, ka ba nyɔɔ wʋ fɩr ka wʋ de a Yesu daa tuo.
41015022	Ba chiin naa a Yesu tɩ tãn a be ban bʋɔlɔ a Yesu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr pɔ, Gɔlgɔta. A par lɛ ɩka, Julaa Jie.
41015023	Ka ba pãa de tɩ̃ɩ kɔ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a dãa pɔ, ɩka wʋ nyũ, tɩ wʋ tɔr.
41015024	Be lɛ ba kpa wʋ a daa ju. Ba põ naa a wʋ fɔɔr na ba ŋme gbãm bɔ̃ɔ a ala ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na na de.
41015025	Bibipɔl lɛ ba kpa wʋ.
41015026	Ba sɛb naa a yele 'lɔ jũu ban kʋn wʋ mar a daa jũu ɩka, "A JUU NƖBƐ NÃA."
41015027	Ba mɩ kpan nãnyisɩ ayi a dabãbɩ̃nsɩ mɩ ju, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ be a Yesu nũsʋ̃ɔ loor ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ be a wʋ gʋba loor.
41015029	A bala na tala a be a wʋ kpafʋ jie tʋrɔ wʋ, vavire a ba jur 'yɛrɛ, "Wooo, a fʋ̃ʋ nyã na 'yɛr ɩka fʋn sɔ̃ɔ naa a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ Yir nyã bar tɩ mɛ wʋ a ber ata,
41015030	wa suu a daa ju, na fʋ faa a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ!"
41015031	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ, a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe mɩ laara wʋ, na ba 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Nyɛ, wʋ faan bamɩne, tɩ wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ faa ɛ!
41015032	Vɛ̃ a 'lɔ na 'yɛr ɩka, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa, na wʋ ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ nãa, suu a daa ju a sɩ kaa, tɩ na sɩ pãa sɔɔ." A bala mɩ ban kpa gbʋr wʋ, lɛ lɛ ba mɩ tʋ wʋ.
41015033	A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa ara a gar ju sãlsɔɔ, a wɛr wʋ jaa sɔb naa wa tɩ tãn a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ balfʋ sɔ̃ɔ.
41015034	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ lɛ, ka a Yesu chɩɩr bʋɔl, "Eloi, eloi, lama sabakatanɩ." A par lɛ a Yesu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr pɔ ɩka, "N Nãaŋmɩn, n Nãaŋmɩn, bo lɛ so ka fʋ lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ ma?"
41015035	A bala na ara gbʋr a be wõ na ba 'yɛr, "Yɩ chɛlɛ! Elaija lɛ wʋ bʋɔlɔ."
41015036	Ka a daba ɩ̃sʋɔ jo chen tɩ 'mɔɔ sapɔ 'lɔr a dãmiir amɩne pɔ, na wʋ chab daa tur a Yesu ɩka wʋ mʋʋr, tɩ na wʋ lɛ 'yɛr, "Yɩ vɛ̃ a sɩ kaara, Elaija na wa yɔɔ wʋ naa bɩɩ."
41015037	Be lɛ a Yesu chɩɩr tɩ ŋmaa a vʋʋr.
41015038	Ka a Juu Nɩbɛ Puorfʋ Yir pɔ, ban lũ a fɔbaa var a die chɩɛr a saaju tɩ gbem a par.
41015039	A sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na ara a be a Yesu niem na wõ a wʋ chɩɩrfʋ, tɩ nyɛ a lɛ mɩ wʋn ŋmaa a vʋʋr, wʋ 'yɛr naa, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa, a daba nyã ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn Bie."
41015040	A pɔbɔ bamɩne lɔ̃ɔn Mɛɛr na yi Magdala tẽe pɔ, nɩ Salome, nɩ a Mɛɛr na ɩ a Jemesɩ bile, nɩ Josesɩ ma mɩ ara na tɛɛr jaa tɩ kaar wʋ.
41015041	A Galilee pɔ, a pɔbɔ banyãna lɛ turo wʋ, na ba sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ. Ka a pɔbɔ bamɩne mɩ na 'matãan wʋ wa a Jerusalɛm, mɩ be be.
41015042	A daar 'lɔ ɩ naa a ba Chɔɔrfʋ Bɩbir ban na chɔɔr a ba mɩ̃ɛ, bojũu a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ wa mʋr, a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir piel naa. A jãanʋɔr na wa tara
41015043	a Josefʋ na yi a Arimatɩya tẽe pɔ, na ɩ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ ban 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃, tɩ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ chɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Nãalʋ̃ʋ, nyɔɔn nyãa chen a Pilate sɛ̃, tɩ sʋɔr a Yesu ɩ̃gãn ɩka wʋ ũu.
41015044	Pilate na wa wõ ɩka a Yesu kpi naa, a 'maa wʋn nɛɛ. Be lɛ wʋ bʋɔl a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ka wʋ wa, ka wʋ sʋʋr wʋ, "A Yesu kpin bɩɩ?"
41015045	Ka a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, wʋ kpi naa." Ka a Pilate sɔɔ ɩka a Josefʋ wʋ tɩ yɔɔ a Yesu ɩ̃gãn.
41015046	Josefʋ dãn fɔbaa na wʋ tɩ yɔɔ a Yesu ɩ̃gãn vil wʋ chiin tɩ ũu, a yaa ban chɩ kʋsɩr pɔ. Ba bil kʋsɩr wa pɔɔ a yaa nɛɛ.
41015047	A Mɛɛr na yi a Magdala, nɩ a Mɛɛr na ɩ a Josesɩ ma, nyɛ naa a jie 'lɔ ban ũu wʋ.
41016001	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir na wa baar, Mɛɛr na yi a Magdala, nɩ Salome, nɩ a Mɛɛr na ɩ a Jemesɩ ma, ba dãn a kãnyũur ala ɩka ba chiin tɩ jɛ a Yesu ɩ̃gãn.
41016002	A Pɛ̃nfʋ divɩɛ bio daar, bibio mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na pur baar, ba chen naa a yaa par.
41016003	A kʋsɩr na pɔɔ a yaa nɛɛ ba gbʋr ɛ, ka ba sʋrɔ taa, "An lɛ na tɩ bil a kʋsɩr bar sɩ a yaa nɛɛ?"
41016004	Tɩchɛ ban dʋɔ kaa a ba nidaa, a kʋsɩr 'lɔ bil yi a yaa nɛɛ.
41016005	Ban tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a yaa pɔ, ba nyɛn pɔlbile na su fuu pɩla jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a nũsʋ̃ɔ loor, ka pɩla ɔɔ ba.
41016006	A pɔlbile 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka yɩ pɩla ɔɔrɔ ɛ. Yɩ bʋɔrɔ naa a Yesu 'lɔ na yi a Najaretɩ ban kpa a daa ju. Wʋ ir naa ɩ vʋr! Waa be a ka ɛ! Yɩ nyɛ a jie 'lɔ ban gaal wʋ.
41016007	Yɩ lɩɛb kul tɩ 'yɛr a wʋ poturbo nɩ a Pita ɩka, wʋ de yɩn nie chiine a Galilee, be lɛ yɩn tɩ nyɛ wʋ, nɩtãa a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ."
41016008	Chĩcham kpɛ ba naa ka ba nɛɛ 'maa, ka ba jo yi a yaa par. Baa 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ, bojũu dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba naa.
41016009	A Pɛ̃nfʋ divɩɛ bio daar bibio, Yesu na wa ir a kũu pɔ, wʋ den nie dũu a Mɛɛr na yi a Magdala, a 'lɔ pɔ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ dii a sɩdɛbɛ ayopõi bar ka a yi.
41016010	A Mɛɛr chen tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a bala na dɔ̃ɔ be a Yesu sɛ̃, a bala a nie na sɔb ka baa kõnõ.
41016011	Ban wa wõ ka wʋ 'yɛr ɩka a Yesu ir naa kũu pɔ ɩ vʋr, ka wʋ nyɛ wʋ, baa sɔɔ de ɛ.
41016012	A anyã puor lɛ, a Yesu lɩɛb nɩyuo na wʋ dũu a ba ayi na de sɔr chiine a tẽe ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ.
41016013	Ba lɩɛb chen a Jerusalɛm tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a ba taaba, tɩchɛ baa sɔɔ ɛ.
41016014	A ba kor ɛ, tɩ a Yesu lɛ dũu a Pie nɩ Bʋ̃'yen na 'mataa dire. Wʋ miin 'yɔ̃ɔ ba a ba ba sɔɔfʋ pɔ, nɩ a ba nyãkpɩ̃ɛn jũu, bojũu baa sɔɔ de a bala na nyɛ wʋn ir a kũu pɔ 'yɛr.
41016015	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ yɔ a wɛr wʋ jaa, na yɩ mʋɔl 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã kʋ a nɩbʋrɔ ba jaa.
41016016	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã, ka ba so wʋ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, wʋn nyɛn a Nãaŋmɩn faafʋ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ba sɔɔ de a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã ɛ, a nɩnyɩnɛ na wɛ naa.
41016017	A jɩ̃nsɩ anyã na turo naa bala na sɔɔ. Ban de naa n yuor diin sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi, na ba lɛ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛrbʋlsɩ 'yɛrfʋ.
41016018	Ban ma 'mɔɔr waba. Bala wa nyũ bon na tara lɔɔ, tɩ a kʋ̃ ɩ ba yele ɛ. Baalaa ban dɔɔl a ba nũu, wʋn sa naa."
41016019	A Soro Yesu na wa 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ kʋ a wʋ poturbo, Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃ naa ka wʋ do a saaju tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ loor.
41016020	Be lɛ ka a poturbo yi chen tɩ mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ jie jaa. Be lɛ ka a Soro 'mataa tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ ba, ka a wʋ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ anyã ban tʋ̃nɔ̃ wiil ɩka a wʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ.
42001001	Nɩtãa lɛ a nɩyɔɔ na mɔ̃ man a lɛ na ɩ a sɩ ber anyã pɔ,
42001002	a lɛ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ, ba dɔ̃ɔ be be na ba nyɛn nɩbir a pielfʋ, na ba ɩ a 'yɛr nyã gbãgbaar.
42001003	A lɛ jũu n baraa Teofilusɩ, n mɩ mɔ̃n vɩɛr a 'yɛr tɩ tãn a pielfʋ nyɛ ka a ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ, ka n bʋɔrɔ ɩka n sɛb a lɛ na tu taa kʋ fʋ.
42001004	Ka fʋ na tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a lɛ ban wiil fʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ.
42001005	A Judiya Nãa Hɛrɔd sɔ̃ɔ, a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrloro ɩ̃sʋɔ ben be ban bʋɔlɔ Jekariya wʋ pʋɔ naa a Abija gbul pɔ ka a wʋ pɔɔ yuor di Elijabetɩ na yi a Aaron bʋrɔ pɔ.
42001006	Ba jaa ayi yele tor Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ka ba turo a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ na 'yɛr na baa tara chɛfʋ ɛ.
42001007	Tɩchɛ baa tara bie ɛ, bojũu a Elijabetɩ abbaa ka 'lɔ naa sɩrɛ jaa nyɔ̃ɔ.
42001008	A mɩ lʋɔr wa ta a Jekariya ka wʋ̃n tʋ̃ a bɔɔr lofʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn.
42001009	Gbãm lɛ ba gba ir wʋ nɩtãa lɛ a ba bɔɔrlo tʋ̃mɔ̃ na be, ka wʋn ma kpɛ a puorfʋ yir tɩ chʋm a tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla ala.
42001010	Ka a sɔ̃ɔ na wa ta ɩka wʋ chʋm a tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla anyãna, a nɩbɛ ara naa a yõo puoro.
42001011	Be lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn malaka wa dũu wʋ be a tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla chʋmfʋ jie a nũsʋ̃ɔ jie.
42001012	Jekariya na wa nyɛ wʋ a lɛ, pɩla ɔɔ wʋ naa ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ wʋ.
42001013	Tɩchɛ ka a malaka 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Jekariya ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn wõn a fʋ sʋɔrfʋ, a fʋ pɔɔ Elijabetɩ na dɔɔn dabile ka fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ yuor Jɔɔn.
42001014	A wʋ yele na ɩn nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ fʋ ka fʋ chɩlɛ ka nɩyɔɔ mɩ chɩlɛ a wʋ dɔɔfʋ jũu.
42001015	An ɩ wʋn ɩn kpɛ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn niem, wʋ kʋ̃ nyũ dãa ban 'yɔ̃ɔ dãbɩl ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na sɛɛ wʋn be a ma pʋɔm.
42001016	Wʋn lɩɛb naa a Isɩral nɩbɛ yɔɔ jie waan a ba Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
42001017	Wʋn den a sɩ Soro nie nɩ a sɩɛ nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ be a Elaija 'yɔ̃ɔ, na wʋ lɩɛb sãamɩne ka ba tara a ba bibiir tɩɛr. Ka bawõnsɩ mɩ nyɛ yɛ̃ na ba maala yeltorsɩ na wʋ vɛ̃ ka nɩbɛ mɩ chɔɔr ba mɩ̃ɛ gun a sɩ Soro."
42001018	Ka a Jekariya sʋʋr a malaka, "Ŋmɩnɛ ɩn ɩrɛ wa sɔɔ a nɩtɔ̃ fʋn 'yɛr? Maa nɩ n pɔɔ jaa kor naa."
42001019	Ka a malaka 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Maa lɛ a Gabɩrɛl na ma ara a Nãaŋmɩn niem, 'lɔ lɛ tʋ̃ ma nɩ a 'yɛr nyã ɩka n wa 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã kʋ fʋ.
42001020	A lɛ jũu fʋn ɩn wõo fʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr 'yɛr ɛ, wa tãn a bɩbir 'lɔ a anyãna na ɩ bojũu faa sɔɔ de a 'yɛr ala na wa ɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ na sɛɛ ɛ."
42001021	A nɩbɛ bala na be a yõo chɛlɛ a Jekariya wʋ̃n kor a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir, ka chĩcham kpɛ ba.
42001022	Be lɛ ka wʋ wa yi tɩ wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr 'yɛr ɛ, ka a nɩbɛ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka wʋ nyɛn nyɛfʋ kɔ̃ɔ bojũu nuur kaalfʋ lɛ wʋ mana nɩ ba tɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɛ.
42001023	A lɛ a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ bɩbie na wa baar be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir, wʋ lɩɛb kul a wʋ yir.
42001024	A anyã puor lɛ ka wʋ pɔɔ Elijabetɩ tara pʋɔ na wʋ sɔɔl ŋmɛrsɩ anũu.
42001025	Na wʋ pãa 'yɛrɛ, "Nyɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na maal ma, a wʋ maal vɩla bɩbir vɩɛ naa ka wʋ ir ma a vĩ yin a nɩbɛ niem bar."
42001026	Elijabetɩ pʋɔ na wa ta ŋmɛrsɩ ayʋɔb, Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃ naa a Gabɩrɛl a tẽe na be a Galilee paal pɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Najaretɩ,
42001027	be lɛ pɔɔsarbile kɔ̃ɔ be, ka daba ban bʋɔlɔ Josefʋ na ɩ a Nãa David yɔ̃ɔ ŋmaa baraa na kul ka a pɔɔbile yuor di Mɛɛr.
42001028	A malaka chen a wʋ sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "N puorfʋ naa, fʋ ɩn nɩ'yɔ̃ɔ naa, Nãaŋmɩn ben a fʋ sɛ̃."
42001029	Ka dãbɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔ a Mɛɛr nɩ a puorfʋ nyã bʋrɔ, na wʋ sʋrɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a puorfʋ nyã par.
42001030	Tɩchɛ ka a malaka 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, fʋ ɩn nɩ'yɔ̃ɔ naa Nãaŋmɩn niem.
42001031	Fʋn tara na pʋɔ dɔɔ dabile, na fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ yuor Yesu.
42001032	Wʋn ɩn kpɛ̃ɛ, ka ba bʋɔlɔ wʋ a Nãaŋmɩn na be a Saaju Bie. A sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn na den a wʋ sãa David nãalʋ̃ʋ kʋ wʋ.
42001033	'Lɔ lɛ na di a Jekɔb yir nãa jaa kpo kpo, a wʋ nãa kʋ̃ wa baar ɛ."
42001034	Ka a Mɛɛr sʋʋr a malaka, "N ba ta daba sɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ ŋmɩnɛ ɩn ɩrɛ wa dɔɔ a bie?"
42001035	Ka a malaka 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na wa kpɛ fʋ naa, ka a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ wa ger pɔɔ fʋ a bichɛchɛ 'lɔ fʋn na dɔɔ, ban bʋɔlɔ wʋ̃n Nãaŋmɩn Bie.
42001036	Nyɛ a fʋ yɛbɛ Elijabetɩ gba na ɩ a pɔɔ abbaa na wʋ nyɔ̃ɔ tɩ wʋ tara na pʋɔ na dɔɔ bie, chuur ayʋɔb nɩ nyã wʋn gal.
42001037	Yele jaa ba ɩ tuo Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ."
42001038	Be lɛ a Mɛɛr 'yɛr, "Nyɛ, Nãaŋmɩn gbãgbaa lɛ n ɩ, a ɩ a lɛ kʋ ma fʋn 'yɛr?" Ka a malaka bar wʋ tɩ chen.
42001039	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a Mɛɛr pɔɔ yi do a tɔ̃ɔ ju a Judiya tẽe pɔ.
42001040	Wʋ tɩ kpɛ naa a Jekariya yir na wʋ puor a Elijabetɩ.
42001041	Elijabetɩ na wõ a Mɛɛr puorfʋ ka a bie ɔɔ lɩɛb be a wʋ pʋɔm ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛɛ a Elijabetɩ.
42001042	Ka wʋ ŋme chɛlma 'yɛrɛ, "Nãaŋmɩn sʋ̃ʋ fʋn gar a pɔbɔ ba jaa, na wʋ mɩ sʋ̃ʋ a bie 'lɔ na be a fʋ pʋɔm.
42001043	Tɩchɛ nyɛ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ na kaara, ka a n Soro ma wa a n sɛ̃?
42001044	Ɩ̃n wa wõ a fʋ puorfʋ a bie na gã a n pʋɔm ɔɔn lɩɛb nɩ pʋpɛl.
42001045	Pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ fʋ ɩ an ɩ fʋ sɔɔn de a lɛ a n Soro na tʋ̃, ka ba wa 'yɛr fʋ ɩka an ɩ naa a lɛ."
42001046	Ka a Mɛɛr 'yɛr, "N pɛɛn Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a pʋɔ wʋ jaa.
42001047	A n sɩɛ chɩlɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a n Fafaara 'yɔ̃ɔ.
42001048	An ɩ wʋ tɩɛrtɔ a wʋ gbãgbapɔɔbile mɩ̃ɛ siirfʋ. An yi dɩna chiine, a dɔɔ tu taa ba jaa na bʋɔlɔ ma naa bɔɔsʋ̃n sʋɔ.
42001049	An ɩ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ lɛ maal a lɛ kʋ ma. A wʋ yuor ɩn chɛchɛ.
42001050	A wʋ nɩbaal be naa a bala na joro wʋ dãbɩ̃ɛ sɛ̃, yi a yɔn tɩ tãn a yɔn suulsɩ.
42001051	A wʋ nũu tʋ̃n tʋ̃bɛrɛ, wʋ yɛ̃yɛl naa a bala na bʋɔrɔ a yuor a ba tɩɛr pɔ bar.
42001052	Wʋ dɔɔn nãmɩne a ba nãa dakɔɔr jur bar, tɩchɛ na wʋ 'mɔɔr a bala na siir a ba mɩ̃ɛ ka ba do saaju.
42001053	Wʋ kʋ naa a kɔ̃ dẽme bʋ̃sʋ̃n, tɩ dii a tara dẽme bar nũjaalsɩ.
42001054	Wʋ sʋ̃ʋn a wʋ gbãgbaa Isɩral tɩ tɩɛrtɔ ɩka wʋ kaa Abraham nɩ a wʋ yɔn nɩbaal bɩbir jaa, nɩtãa lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a sɩ sãamɩne."
42001056	Mɛɛr jɩ̃nɛ na a Elijabetɩ sɛ̃ ŋmɛrsɩ ata tɩ lɩɛb kul a wʋ tẽe.
42001057	Elijabetɩ dɔɔfʋ bɩbir wa vɩɛ naa ka wʋ dɔɔ dabile.
42001058	Ka a bala na kpɩɛrɛ gbʋr a Elijabetɩ nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme na wõ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na maal vɩla kʋ wʋ ba pʋɔ mɩ pɛl naa a wʋ kaar.
42001059	A ber aniin daar ba wa naa ɩka ba wa ŋmaa a bie yʋɔr, na ba ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba de a sãa yuor 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ bʋɔlɔ a Jekariya.
42001060	Tɩchɛ ka a ma ba sɔɔ ɛ, tɩ 'yɛr, "A bie yuor din Jɔɔn."
42001061	A ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Fʋ bal nɩrɛ jaa ba di a yuor nyã ɛ."
42001062	Tɩ na ba pãa 'lɩɩr sʋʋr a sãa a yobuor wʋn bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a bie.
42001063	Ka wʋ man ba ɩka ba kʋ wʋ bon ka wʋ sɛb, wʋn ben wa de a bon na wʋ sɛb, "A bie yuor din Jɔɔn." Ka nɛɛr 'maa ba jaa.
42001064	Ajienaa lɛ a Jekariya nɛɛ mɩ 'laa ka a jãlbir bal ka wʋ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ na wʋ pɛɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn.
42001065	Ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a bala jaa na gbʋr a be ka nɩbɛ 'yɛrɛ ka a yaar de a Judiya tẽn ala na be a tɔ̃n ju.
42001066	Nɩrɛ jaa na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ a ma 'maa wʋn nɛɛ ka wʋ ma sʋʋr, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a bie nyã na wa kaara?" Bojũu a Soro nũu dɔɔl naa a bie.
42001067	Jekariya na ɩ a sãa, Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛɛ wʋ naa ka wʋ 'yɛrɛ,
42001068	"Pɛɛfʋ wʋ ta a Isɩral Nãaŋmɩn, bojũu wʋ wa naa wa faa a wʋ nɩbɛ.
42001069	Wʋ kʋ sɩn gãdaa ɩka wʋ faa sɩ na yi a wʋ gbãgbaa Nãa David yir,
42001070	nɩtãa lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ tu a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ chɛchɛ bala sɛ̃ a kõr jaa ka ba 'yɛr,
42001071	ɩka wʋ faa sɩ a sɩ dɔ̃dẽme sɛ̃, na wʋ faa sɩ a bala na laar sɩ nuur pɔ.
42001072	Wʋ maal a nɩtɔ̃ ɩka wʋ wiil nɩbaal kʋ a sɩ sãamɩne, na wʋ lɛ tɩɛr a wʋ nɛtɩr chɛchɛ 'lɔ,
42001073	a lɛ wʋn pɔ kʋ a sɩ sãakpã Abraham.
42001074	Wʋ pɔn 'yɛr ɩka, wʋn faa sɩ naa a sɩ dɔ̃dẽme nuur pɔ, ka sɩ puoro wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ,
42001075	na sɩ ɩ chɛchɛ nɩ nɩtorsɩ a wʋ niem a ber a jaa.
42001076	A fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ a n bie ban bʋɔlɔ fʋ naa a saaju Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ, an ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ na de a sɩ Soro nie chɔɔr a wʋ sɔr,
42001077	na fʋ vɛ̃ ka wʋ nɩbɛ bɔ̃ɔ a faafʋ sɔr, na ba nyɛ yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ.
42001078	Nãaŋmɩn na tara nɩ sɩ nɩbaal jũu, wʋ vɛ̃ naa ka a fafaara pur chaar 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ yi a saaju,
42001079	na wʋ chaar 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na kpɩɛrɛ a libe pɔ, tɩ be a kũu gãagiel pĩlem, na wʋ wiil a sɩ gbɛɛ ka a de nyã'maar sɔr."
42001080	A bie nʋ̃ɔ naa ka a sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ be a wʋ sɛ̃. Mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ lɛ wʋ kpɩɛrɛ tɩ tãn a bɩbir 'lɔ wʋn na wiil a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Isɩral nɩbɛ.
42002001	A ber ala pɔ, a paal Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa Agustus 'yɛr naa ɩka ba sɔr a nɩbɛ ba jaa na be a Worom paal pɔ.
42002002	A sɔrfʋ nyã lɛ ɩ a sɔrdɔ̃ɔ ban sɔr a nɩbɛ ka a Kiriniyus mɩ ɩ a Siriya nãa.
42002003	Nɩrɛ jaa kul a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tẽe ka ban tɩ sɔr wʋ.
42002004	Ala lɛ so ka a Josefʋ mɩ na yi a Najaretɩ tẽe na be a Galilee wɛr pɔ, na wʋ chen a Judiya wɛr pɔ, a Nãa David tẽe ban bʋɔlɔ a Bɛtɩlɛhɛm, bojũu a Nãa David yir lɛ wʋ yi tɩ lɛ ɩ a wʋ bal nɩrɛ.
42002005	Josefʋ tara na a Mɛɛr na tara a pʋɔ wʋn bʋɔrɔ a kulfʋ 'mataa chiin ka ban tɩ sɔr ba.
42002006	A lɛ ban be a Bɛtɩlɛhɛm ka a Mɛɛr bie dɔɔfʋ daar ta.
42002007	Ka wʋ dɔɔ a pɔɔsarbie ka wʋ ɩ dabile a wʋ vil wʋ a fɔbaa gaal a dʋ̃n mʋɔr 'wɔfʋ jie bojũu baa nyɛ jie na kpɛ a sãanba kpɛfʋ jie ɛ.
42002008	Pɛchiinbɛ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ gbʋr a tẽe na ba gãn a ba piir be a mʋ̃ɔ pɔ kaara.
42002009	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn malaka yi a saaju wa a ba sɛ̃, ka Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr chaar pɔɔ ba, ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba.
42002010	Tɩchɛ a malaka 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ lɛ n waan a yɩ sɛ̃, an ɩn chɩlfʋ kpɛ̃ɛ kʋ a nɩbɛ ba jaa.
42002011	A dɩna tɩ̃sɔɔ ba dɔɔ naa a Fafaara a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãa David tẽe pɔ. Wʋ ɩ naa a sɩ Soro nɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
42002012	Jɩ̃nɛ yɩn na de bɔ̃ɔn wʋ nɩ nyã. Yɩn nyɛ naa a bipɩla ban vil a fɔbaa gaal wʋ a dʋ̃n mʋɔr 'wɔfʋ jie."
42002013	Ajienaa a saaju malakasɩ yɔɔ wa naa wa 'matãan a malaka 'lɔ a ba dãna a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ nɩ,
42002014	"Tɩɩr wʋ ta a Nãaŋmɩn na be a saaju, ka nyã'maar mɩ be a nɩbɛ bala na pɛlɛ a wʋ pʋɔ a wɛr pɔ."
42002015	A malakasɩ na wa bar ba tɩ lɩɛb do a saaju, ka a pɛchiinbɛ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Yɩ ɩ a sɩ chen a Bɛtɩlɛhɛm tẽe pɔ, tɩ kaa a yelnyɩnɛ na ɩ ka a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃ 'yɛr sɩ."
42002016	Be lɛ ba pɔɔ chen tɩ nyɛ a Mɛɛr nɩ a Josefʋ nɩ a bipɩla na gã a dʋ̃n mʋɔr 'wɔfʋ jie.
42002017	A lɛ ban wa nyɛ wʋ, ba 'yɛr naa a lɛ a malaka na 'yɛr kʋ ba a bibile yele.
42002018	A bala ba jaa na wõ a lɛ a pɛchiinbɛ na 'yɛr a bie 'yɛr kʋ ba, ka nɛɛr 'maa ba jaa.
42002019	Tɩchɛ ka a Mɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a anyãna a wʋ pʋɔm tara tɩɛrɛ.
42002020	A pɛchiinbɛ lɩɛb chen a piir jie tɩ dãna Nãaŋmɩn na ba pɛɛrɛ wʋ a ala a jaa ban wõ tɩ nyɛ a lɛ a malaka na 'yɛr kʋ ba.
42002021	A ber aniin na wa ta, ba ŋmaa wʋn a yʋɔr tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ a yuor Yesu, a yuor nyã lɛ a malaka 'yɛr kʋ a Mɛɛr tɩ ka wʋ wa tara a pʋɔ.
42002022	Mɛɛr na wa baar a padɔɔr a lɛ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ na 'yɛr, Josefʋ nɩ a Mɛɛr den a bie chiin a Jerusalɛm na tɩ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn.
42002023	Nɩtãa lɛ a Soro na 'yɛr, "Yɩ de dabil dɔ̃ɔ jaa kʋ a Soro."
42002024	Ba den a bɔɔrlo bomo ala a Soro na 'yɛr ɩka, "Ŋmama ayi bɩɩ papa pɔlɔ ayi tɩ pɔl a ba mɩ̃ɛ."
42002025	Daba kɔ̃ɔ dɔ̃ɔ be a Jerusalɛm ban bʋɔlɔ Simeon na wʋ ɩ nɩtor na waa baala Nãaŋmɩn ɛ. Wʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ chɛlɛ a Isɩral nɩbɛ faafʋ bɩbir ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ be a wʋ sɛ̃.
42002026	A Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ɩka wʋn nyɛ naa a Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ a Soro na tʋ̃ nɩ nɩbir tɩ kpi.
42002027	A Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ vɛ̃n ka Simeon chen be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, ka a ɩ a Josefʋ nɩ a Mɛɛr mɩ waan naa a ba bie Yesu a be na wa ir a nɛɛ.
42002028	Ka a Simeon de a bie 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ nũu pɔ tɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan 'yɛrɛ,
42002029	"Tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋɔ, nɩtãa lɛ fʋn tɩr a fʋ nɛɛ kʋ a maa na ɩ a fʋ gbãgbaa, fʋn tʋ̃ɔ bar ma sɔr nɩ nyã'maar.
42002030	Bojũu n nɩbir nyɛ naa a fafaara,
42002031	'lɔ fʋn chɔɔr ka nɩrɛ jaa nyɛ wʋ.
42002032	Wʋn ɩn chãa wiil a nɩbɛ bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, tɩ na wʋ ɩ tɩɩr kʋ a fʋ nɩbɛ Isɩral."
42002033	Ka a Yesu sãa nɩ a ma nɛɛ 'maa a lɛ a Simeon na 'yɛr a wʋ yele.
42002034	Ka a Simeon pãa 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ ba, tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Mɛɛr na ɩ a ma, "A bie nyãna lɛ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ a Isɩral nɩbɛ, ka ba yɔɔ na ŋme gbɛr lo tɩ ir, na wʋ ɩ jɩ̃nɛ ka ban 'yɛrɛ kpɛrɛ nɩ wʋ.
42002035	Nɩbɛ yɔɔ pʋtɩɛr na gãn chãa pɔ, ka a fʋ̃ʋ mɩ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ fɩka sʋɔ ban chɔr fʋ."
42002036	Pɔɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ben be ban bʋɔlɔ Ana na wʋ ɩ Fanuwɛl bie na wʋ ɩ Aserɩ bal nɩrɛ, na wʋ ɩ pɔɔ nyɔ̃ɔ. Wʋ kul sɩrɛ maal yuomo ayopõi.
42002037	Ka a sɩrɛ kpi tɩ wʋ ɩ a pɔɔkʋɔr maal yuomo lɩjaanaar nɩ anaar (84). Waa gala a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ma ben be na wʋ ma gal bʋ̃diir tɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn tɩ̃sɔɔ nɩ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ.
42002038	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ wʋ wa a ba sɛ̃ tɩ dãn Nãaŋmɩn tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr a bie 'yɛr kʋ a bala jaa na chɛlɛ a Jerusalɛm faafʋ bɩbir.
42002039	A lɛ a Josefʋ nɩ a Mɛɛr na wa ir a nɛɛ maal a lɛ a Soro na bin, ba lɩɛb kul a Najaretɩ na ɩ a ba tẽe na be a Galilee wɛr pɔ.
42002040	Be lɛ a bie tɩ nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ fɔ̃ɔ na wʋ sɛɛn yɛ̃ ka a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ be a wʋ sɛ̃.
42002041	Yuon jaa a sãa naa ma ma chen a Jerusalɛm tɩ lɔ̃ɔ na ba di a Gõl Bar Difʋ.
42002042	Yesu na wa nyɛ yuomo pie nɩ ayi ba tara wʋn don a Difʋ nyã jie nɩtãa lɛ ban ma ɩrɛ.
42002043	A Gõl Bar Difʋ ber na wa baar, ba lɩɛb kulo a ba tẽe tɩchɛ a Yesu bar a Jerusalɛm ka baa bɔ̃ɔn ɛ.
42002044	Ba tɩɛr ɩka wʋ taa pɔɔ a ba nɩbɛ kulo nɩ tɩ chen bɩbir bʋ̃'yen baa nyɛ wʋ ɛ, na ba pãa yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ wʋ a ba nɩbɛ nɩ a ba nɩbɔ̃ɔnsɩ nɩ a ba barmɩne sɛ̃.
42002045	Ban ba wa nyɛ wʋ ɛ, ba lɩɛb chen a Jerusalɛm a wʋ bɔfʋ jie.
42002046	A ber ata daar lɛ a ba tɩ nyɛ wʋ a be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, ka wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a wiwiilbe chara pɔ chɛlɛ a lɛ ban 'yɛrɛ na wʋ sʋrɔ ba sʋʋrfʋsɩ.
42002047	Nɩrɛ jaa na wõ a lɛ wʋn ire a 'yɛrsɩ par a chɔ̃ chɔ̃ nɛɛ 'maa ba naa.
42002048	A sãa nɩ a ma na wa nyɛ wʋ a ba nɛɛ mɩ 'maa ba naa ka a ma sʋʋr, "Pa n bie, bo lɛ fʋ maal sɩ a nɩtɔ̃, ka maa nɩ a fʋ sãa yɔbɔ fʋ lɛ̃ɛɛ wa faa?"
42002049	Ka Yesu sʋʋr a ma, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ ma? Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka ɩn be naa a n Sãa yir ɛ?"
42002050	Tɩchɛ baa bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna wʋn 'yɛr kʋ ba par ɛ.
42002051	A wʋ ir pɔɔ ba, a ba pãa kul a Najaretɩ a wʋ tɩ wõnõ a ba toor, tɩchɛ ka a ma 'yɔ̃ɔ a 'yɛr anyãna a jaa a wʋ pʋɔm.
42002052	Ka a Yesu nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ yɛ̃ nɩ a kpɛ̃ɛ ka wʋ yele nʋ̃mɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ nɩ a nɩbɛ sɛ̃.
42003001	Yuon pie nɩ anũu lɛ a Tiberiyus Siisa di a nãkpɛ̃ɛ ka a Pontius Pilate mɩ ɩ a Judiya paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ka a Hɛrɔd mɩ di a Galilee nãa ka a wʋ yɛbɛ Filip mɩ ɩ a Ituriya nɩ a Tɩrakonɩtɩs nãa. Ka a Lisaniyasɩ mɩ di a Abilenɩ nãa.
42003002	Anasɩ nɩ Kayafasɩ bala lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ. Ka a Nãaŋmɩn de a wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Jekariya bidaba Jɔɔn be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ.
42003003	Wʋ yɔn a tẽn ala a jaa na jilʋ̃ a Jordan man na wʋ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ, "Yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr na yɩ so a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ka Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃ a yɩ yeldɛbɛ kʋ yɩ."
42003004	Nɩtãa lɛ a Isaiya na sɛb a wʋ gãn pɔ, "Nɩrɛ 'yɛrɛ naa be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ, 'Yɩ chɔɔr a sɩ Soro sɔr, na yɩ maal a wʋ sɔr ka wʋ tor.
42003005	Na yɩ 'mʋr a kʋlsɩ, na yɩ ŋmɛr a tɔ̃n nɩ a gbẽgbẽnsɩ ka a jɩ̃taa. Yɩ maal a sɔgɔ̃rsɩ a jaa ka a tor, na yɩ maal a sɔr nyara nyara ka wʋ sal.
42003006	Nɩsaal bʋrɔ ba jaa na nyɛn Nãaŋmɩn faafʋ.' "
42003007	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na waara a Jɔɔn sɛ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Yɩn waa bibiir, an lɛ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka yɩ jo yi a Nãaŋmɩn suur na waara a yɩ sɛ̃?
42003008	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka yɩ befʋ wiil ɩka yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr. Yɩ ta chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɩka, Abraham lɛ ɩ a sɩ sãa, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ɔn maal a kusɩbɛ anyãna a ba lɩɛb ɩ a Abraham bibiir.
42003009	A 'lar dɔɔl a tɩɛ nyɩbɛ ju, tɩɛ jaa ba wa wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃ sʋ̃n ɛ, ban ŋmaa wʋn lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ bũu pɔ."
42003010	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala sʋʋr wʋ, "Ŋmɩnɛ sɩn pãa ɩ?"
42003011	Ka Jɔɔn 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na tara fuusɩ ayi, wʋ ir ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ na ba tara ɛ, nyã mɩ na tara bʋ̃diir wʋ ɩ a lɛ."
42003012	Lõpodierbe mɩ wan a Jɔɔn sɛ̃ ɩka wʋ so ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, na ba mɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Wiwile sɩ mɩ ɩ ŋmɩnɛ?"
42003013	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ta ma de dɔɔl a lɛ ban ɩka yɩ de ɛ."
42003014	Sojasɩ bamɩne mɩ wan wa sʋʋr wʋ, "Sɩn mɩ, sɩ ɩ ŋmɩnɛ?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ta fɩr nɩrɛ de libir ɛ, yɩ ta mɩ ŋmaa jir kara dɔɔl nɩrɛ ɛ, na yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ sãyar sɛɛn yɩ."
42003015	Ka a nɩbɛ mɩ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ toor chɛlɛ, pãa tɩɛrɛ ɩka a Jɔɔn lɛ tɔ̃ɔ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
42003016	A Jɔɔn 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Maa 'lɔ kʋ̃ɔ lɛ n suoro yɩ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na gar ma na wa naa, a wʋ nafɔɔr mibe gba, n ba sɛɛ ɩka n for ɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ na de Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nɩ bũu son yɩ.
42003017	A ŋmayɩɛl naa ben a wʋ nũu pɔ, a wʋ na yɩɛl a mʋ̃ɩ a vafʋ jie na wʋ kpaar a bie 'yɔ̃ɔ a boor pɔ tɩ chʋm a sɔ̃sɔɔr nɩ bũu 'lɔ na ba tara kpĩinfʋ bar."
42003018	Jɔɔn kpãa ban nɩ yelyɔɔ na wʋ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ ba.
42003019	Tɩchɛ a nãa Hɛrɔd na de a wʋ yɛbɛ pɔɔ Hɛrɔdiyas kul, Jɔɔn 'yɛr wʋ naa ɩka a ba tara sɔr ka wʋ kul wʋ ɛ, tɩ 'yɛr wʋ a dɛbɛ amɩne wʋn ɩ.
42003020	Hɛrɔd lɛ maal dɛɛr wʋn vɛ̃ ka ba nyɔɔ Jɔɔn tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ.
42003021	Ban ba nyɔɔ a Jɔɔn pɔɔ sɛrɛ ɛ, wʋ so naa a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ na wʋ mɩ so a Yesu a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ. Ka a Yesu sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka a saaju yuo.
42003022	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ de papa ɩ̃gãn suu wa 'mar a Yesu ju, tɩ a kɔkɔr yi be a saaju 'yɛr, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a n Bidanʋ̃naa ka fʋ yele pɛl a n pʋɔ."
42003023	Yesu nyɛn yuon lɩjɛr nɩ pie tɩ piel a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃, ka nɩbɛ tɩɛr ɩka wʋ ɩ naa a Josefʋ bidaba, na ɩ a Heli bidaba,
42003024	Matatɩ bidaba, Levi bidaba, Melki bidaba, Janai bidaba, Josefʋ bidaba,
42003025	Matatiyasɩ bidaba, Amosɩ bidaba, Nahum bidaba, Esili bidaba, Nagai bidaba,
42003026	Maat bidaba, Matatiyasɩ bidaba, Semeyin bidaba, Josekɩ bidaba, Joda bidaba,
42003027	Joanan bidaba, Aresa bidaba, Jerubabel bidaba, Sealtɩɛl bidaba, Neri bidaba,
42003028	Melki bidaba, Adi bidaba, Kosam bidaba, Elmadam bidaba, Erɩ bidaba,
42003029	Josua bidaba, Eliyeja bidaba, Jorim bidaba, Matatɩ bidaba, Levi bidaba,
42003030	Simeon bidaba, Juda bidaba, Josefʋ bidaba, Jonam bidaba, Eliyakim bidaba,
42003031	Melea bidaba, Mena bidaba, Matata bidaba, Natan bidaba, David bidaba,
42003032	Jesɩ bidaba, Obed bidaba, Boajɩ bidaba, Salmon bidaba, Nason bidaba,
42003033	Aminadab bidaba, Aram bidaba, Hejoron bidaba, Perejɩ bidaba, Juda bidaba,
42003034	Jekɔb bidaba, Isaakɩ bidaba, Abraham bidaba, Tera bidaba, Nahor bidaba,
42003035	Serugu bidaba, Wɛru bidaba, Peleg bidaba, Eber bidaba, Sela bidaba,
42003036	Kainan bidaba, Afakadɩ bidaba, Sem bidaba, Nowa bidaba, Lamekɩ bidaba,
42003037	Metusela bidaba, Enok bidaba, Jared bidaba, Mahalaleel bidaba, Kenan bidaba,
42003038	Enosɩ bidaba, Setɩ bidaba, Adama bidaba, Nãaŋmɩn bidaba.
42004001	Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛɛn a Yesu na wʋ lɩɛb wʋ yin a Jordan man jie kpɛ̃n wʋ a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ.
42004002	Be lɛ a tɩɩ bɛɛr wʋ kaa ber lɩjaayi, waa di bon jaa a ber anyãna pɔ ɛ, ka a kɔ̃ kpɛ wʋ.
42004003	A tɩɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, 'yɛr kʋ a kʋsɩbɛ anyãna, ka a lɩɛb bʋ̃diir."
42004004	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ɩka, a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Bʋ̃diir tɛɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kʋ nɩrɛ nyɛvʋr ɛ."
42004005	A tɩɩ lɛ tara wʋn don tɔ̃ɔ ju tɩ wiil wʋ a nãa di jiir a jaa na be ka a wɛr pɔ
42004006	tɩ 'yɛr, "Ɩn kʋ fʋ naa anyãna a jaa fɔ̃ɔ nɩ a ba nãyele, maa lɛ ba de a ba fɔ̃ɔ kʋ, ka n mɩ na de kʋ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa ɩn bʋɔrɔ.
42004007	Ala ɩ, fʋ gbur dumo puor ma fʋ̃ʋ lɛ so."
42004008	Ka Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka fʋ puor, na fʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a 'lɔ tɛɛ."
42004009	A tɩɩ lɛ tara wʋn chiin a Jerusalɛm ka wʋ tɩ do a puorfʋ yir jie 'lɔ na do na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie ɔɔ lo a tẽe,
42004010	bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ naa ka a wʋ malakasɩ wa gu fʋ taa lɛɛ,
42004011	na ba nyɔɔ fʋ nɩ a ba nuur ka a fʋ gbɛr kʋ̃ ŋme kʋsɩr ɛ.' "
42004012	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a tɩɩ, a mɩ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Ta bɛɛr a fʋ Nãaŋmɩn kaa ɛ."
42004013	A tɩɩ na wa baar a bɛɛr kaa anyãna wʋ bar wʋn tɩ chen, tɩ lɛ guro nɩ sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ wʋn lɛ wa nyɛ jie.
42004014	Yesu lɩɛb kul a Galilee nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ ka a wʋ yele yaar a wɛr 'lɔ wʋ jaa.
42004015	Wʋ tɩ wile naa a nɩbɛ a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir ka a nɩrɛ jaa pɛɛrɛ wʋ.
42004016	Yesu lɩɛb chen a Najaretɩ be wʋn nʋ̃ɔ, a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar wʋ tɩ kpɛ̃n a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir an ɩ lɛ lɛ wʋ ma ɩrɛ na wʋ ir ara na wʋn kar gãn.
42004017	Ka ba de Isaiya gãn kʋ wʋ, ka wʋ nyɔɔ 'yɩɛr a jie 'lɔ ban sɛb,
42004018	"Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ be naa a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, bojũu wʋ ir ma naa ɩka n tɩ 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ a nɔ̃n dẽme, naa mɩ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ gbãgbaar ka ban so ba mɩ̃ɛ, naa 'yɛr kʋ jɔ̃n ka ba yuo, naa 'yɛr faa a bala ban gere,
42004019	naa 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn maal vɩla yuon kʋ ba."
42004020	Be lɛ wʋ pilʋ̃ a gãn de kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ tɩ jɩ̃nɛ, ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa na be a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir kpa a nɩbie 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ.
42004021	Ka wʋ piel 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ ba, "Dɩna a lɛ yɩn wõ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, a ɩ naa a lɛ."
42004022	Ba jaa 'yɛrɛ naa a wʋ sʋ̃ 'yɛr ka ba nɛɛr 'maa a 'yɛr vɩɛlsɩ na yire a wʋ nɛɛ pɔ ka ba sʋrɔ taa, "A ba ɩ a Josefʋ bidaba lɛ a nyã ɛ?"
42004023	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, yɩn sʋʋr ma naa nɩ a sʋkpa nyã, 'Tɩtɩlɛ, tɩɩl a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ, maal a ala fʋn maal a Kapenahum ka a fʋ tẽe.' "
42004024	A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, ba maa de Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tẽe pɔ ɛ.
42004025	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka pɔɔkɔyɔɔ ben a Isɩral nɩbɛ wɛr pɔ a Elaija sɔ̃ɔ, a war bũu 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ ŋmaa a yuom ata nɩ ŋmɛrsɩ ayʋɔb a wɛr wʋ jaa.
42004026	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn ba tʋ̃ a Elaija a pɔɔkɔɛ ba nyã ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩ tʋ̃ wʋ a pɔɔkʋɔr na be a Jarefat na be a Sidon wɛr pɔ.
42004027	A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Elisa sɔ̃ɔ, kɔ̃kɔ̃n mɩ ben a Isɩral nɩbɛ wɛr pɔ tɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba sa ɛ, ka Naaman na yi a Siriya wɛr pɔ ba lɛ ɛ."
42004028	A nɩyɔɔ bala na be a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir 'lɔ pɔ, ka suur kpɛ ba jaa.
42004029	Ba ir da wʋ yin a tẽe pɔ don a tɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ju a ba tẽe na mɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba daa wʋ lɔb a tɔ̃ɔ koro pɔ.
42004030	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ fʋɔl yi a nɩyɔɔ bala sãlsɔɔ a lɛ na wʋ chen.
42004031	Be lɛ wʋ suu chen a Kapenahum na be a Galilee wɛr pɔ, ka a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar ka wʋ piel wile a nɩbɛ.
42004032	Ka a wʋ wiilfʋ 'maa ba nɛɛ bojũu a wʋ 'yɛr tara na kpɛ̃ɔ.
42004033	Daba mɩ ben a be a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir na tara a dɛɛr sʋɔ, ka a sɩdɛɛr be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, a wʋ ŋme chɛlma sʋʋr,
42004034	"Ai, a fʋ̃ʋ Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ, bo fʋ bʋɔrɔ ka a sɩ sɛ̃? Fʋ wa naa ɩka fʋ wa sɔ̃ɔ sɩ bar bɩɩ? N bɔ̃ɔ naa a nɩnyɩnɛ fʋn ɩ, fʋ ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nɩchɛchɛ 'lɔ."
42004035	Ka Yesu tãn wʋ, "Pɔɔ a nɛɛ tɩ wa yi a daba 'yɔ̃ɔ." A sɩdɛɛr daan a daba lɔb a nɩbɛ niem tɩ na wʋ yi a daba 'yɔ̃ɔ tɩ waa 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ baal ɛ.
42004036	Ka a nɛɛr 'maa a nɩbɛ ka ba sʋrɔ taa, "Wiilbuor mɩ nɩ nyã? Wʋ den kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ tʋ̃ɔfʋ 'yɛr kʋ a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi."
42004037	Ka a wʋ yele yaar de a tẽn ala na jilʋ̃ a be.
42004038	Yesu yi naa a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir na wʋ chen a Simon yir. Ka ɩ̃gãn tɔ a Simon dɩ̃ɛ ma ka ba sʋɔr a Yesu ɩka wʋ sʋ̃ʋ wʋ.
42004039	Ka wʋ guun ger a pɔɔ na wʋ tãn a ɩ̃gãn tʋl ka wʋ bar a pɔɔ, ka wʋ sa na wʋ ir maal bʋ̃diir kʋ ba.
42004040	A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa mʋrɔ nɩbɛ waan naa ba baalsɩ a Yesu sɛ̃, ka wʋ dɔɔl ba a wʋ nũu na wʋ sãa baal jaa bʋrɔ ban waan.
42004041	Sɩdɛbɛ yin a nɩyɔɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Fʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn Bie." Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu tãn ba ka ba ta 'yɛrɛ ɛ, an ɩ ba bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
42004042	A wɛr na wa chaar Yesu yin tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a jie ɩ̃sʋɔ wʋ yõ, ka a nɩbɛ yɔbɔ wʋ tɩ nyɛ a jie wʋn be ba lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ bar ba tɩ chen ɛ.
42004043	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A sɛɛ naa ɩka n 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr kʋ a tẽn anyã mɩ bojũu a lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃ ma."
42004044	Tɩ na wʋ chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr be a a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie a Juu nɩbɛ tẽe pɔ.
42005001	Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ Yesu be naa a Genesaretɩ man nɛɛ, ka nɩyɔɔ ara jilʋ̃ wʋ chɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr.
42005002	Wʋ nyɛn gborsɩ ayi a gogoro nɛɛ a jɩ̃nyɔɔrbɔ na bar tɩ suu pɛɛrɛ a ba lɔyaarsɩ.
42005003	Ka wʋ kpɛ a gboro ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ na ɩ Simon bon tɩ sʋɔr wʋ ɩka wʋ daa wʋ ka wʋ jãan a gogoro bɩ̃lãa. Wʋ pãa jɩ̃nɛ naa a gboro pɔ tɩ wile a nɩbɛ.
42005004	Wʋn wa baar a 'yɛr ka wʋ 'yɛr a Simon, "Daa a gboro chiin a kɔ̃die pɔ na fʋ tɩ lɔb a fʋ lɔyaar."
42005005	Ka a Simon 'yɛr, "Kpãkpãana, tɩ̃sɔɔ jaa lɛ sɩ lɔb lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ saa nyɔɔ bon ɛ, tɩchɛ fʋn 'yɛr go, ɩn lɔbaa."
42005006	Ban wa lɔb, ba nyɔɔr jɩ̃yɔɔ ka a lɔyaarsɩ ɩrɛ na chɩɛr.
42005007	Ka ba 'lɩɩr a ba taaba na be a gboro ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, ka ba wa sʋ̃ʋ ba. Ba wa naa ka a gborsɩ a jaa ayi wa sɛɛ ka ba ɩrɛ na mʋr.
42005008	Simon Pita na wa nyɛ a lɛ, wʋ lon kpa a Yesu niem tɩ 'yɛr, "N Soro sɛr chen tɩ bar ma yelbe-ɩrɛ lɛ n ɩ."
42005009	A jɩ̃yɔɔ anyã ban nyɔɔr jũu, 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ taaba nɛɛr 'maa naa.
42005010	Lɛ lɛ a Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn na ɩ a Jebedee bibiir na ɩ a Simon taaba. Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a Simon, "Ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, an yi dɩna chiine fʋn nyɔɔrɔ na nɩbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
42005011	Be lɛ ba tɔɔ a gborsɩ waan a gogoro nɛɛ wa bar bomo a jaa tɩ turo a Yesu.
42005012	Yesu na wa be a tẽe ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, daba kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ baal na de a ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa nyɛn a Yesu na wʋ lo kpa tẽe a Yesu niem tɩ sʋɔr wʋ, "N Soro, fʋ̃ʋ sɔɔ, sãa ma."
42005013	Ka Yesu tur a wʋ nũu sɩɩr a daba tɩ 'yɛr, "N sɔɔ naa sa." Ajienaa ka a kɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ baal bar wʋ.
42005014	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Taa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ ɛ, tɩ chen tɩ wiil a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrloro na fʋ ir a nɛɛ 'lɔ a Mosesɩ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ka a di dãasɩɛ ɩka fʋ ɩn nɩsʋ̃."
42005015	Tɩchɛ ka a wʋ yele chɛnɛ ŋme yaar a jie wʋ jaa ka a nɩyɔɔ wa chɛlɛ a wʋ 'yɛr ka wʋ sãa a ba baalsɩ.
42005016	Tɩchɛ wʋ ma chɛnɛ na tɔɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ tɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn.
42005017	Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ Yesu na wile ka a ɩ a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe na yi a Galilee tẽbil a jaa nɩ a Judiya ka bamɩne yi a Jerusalɛm mɩ ben be jɩ̃nɛ. Ka a Soro kʋ a Yesu kpɛ̃ɔ ɩka wʋ sãan baalsɩ.
42005018	Dɔɔr bamɩne tuon nɩrɛ nɩ sɔ̃ɔ a nuur nɩ a gbɛɛ na kpi waan bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba kpɛ̃n wʋ tɩ gaal a Yesu niem.
42005019	Ban ba wa nyɛrɛ sɔr a nɩyɔɔ jũu, ba don naa gar ju tɩ yuo bɔɔ tur bar ka wʋ suun a sɔ̃ɔ a nɩbɛ sãlsɔɔ tɩ gã a Yesu niem.
42005020	Yesu na nyɛ a lɛ ban sɔɔ de, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a baalaa, "N baraa, a fʋ yeldɛbɛ vɛ̃n bar."
42005021	Ka a nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Faraseemɩne pãa jɛ̃ tɩɛrɛ, "An lɛ a nyã na jɩ̃nɛ fere sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn yuor a nɩtɔ̃? An lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ nɩrɛ yelbier vɛ̃ bar ka Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ?"
42005022	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban tɩɛrɛ ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Bo lɛ yɩ tɩɛrɛ a anyã a lɛ a yɩ pʋɔm?
42005023	'Yɛr buor lɛ ɩ kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃? N 'yɛr ɩka a wʋ yeldɛbɛ vɛ̃n bar bɩɩ n 'yɛr ɩka wʋ ir chiine?
42005024	Tɩchɛ nɩtɔ̃ lɛ yɩn bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a maa Nɩsaal Bie tara na kpɛ̃ɔ a wɛr pɔ na vɛ̃ yeldɛbɛ bar." Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a dagbɛrɛ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ nɩ ir 'mɔɔ a fʋ sɔ̃ɔ kulo nɩ."
42005025	Ajienaa ka wʋ vaa ir ara a ba niem, 'mɔɔ a wʋ bʋ̃gãnaa pɛɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn kulo nɩ.
42005026	Ka nɩrɛ jaa nɛɛ 'maa ka ba dãna Nãaŋmɩn. Ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba ka ba 'yɛrɛ, "Sɩ nyɛn yelkal bala dɩna."
42005027	A anyã puor Yesu yin tɩ nyɛ lõpodiere ban bʋɔlɔ Levi na jɩ̃nɛ diere wʋ lõposɩ, ka wʋ bʋɔl wʋ, "Ir turo ma."
42005028	Ka a Levi vaa ir bar bomo a jaa tɩ turo wʋ.
42005029	Levi maal bʋ̃diir kʋ a Yesu a be a wʋ yir na wʋ bʋɔl a taaba lõpodierbe nɩ nɩyɔɔ ka ba wa 'mataa dire.
42005030	Tɩchɛ a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe hũhũnõ nɩ a yele nyã sʋrɔ a Yesu poturbo, "Bo lɛ so ka yɩ 'mataa dire nɩ a lõpodierbe nɩ a tʋ̃dɛbɛ tʋ̃nbɔ?"
42005031	Ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A ba ɩ nɩrɛ na kpɛ̃mɛ lɛ chiine tɩtɩlɛ jie ɛ, tɩchɛ baalaa lɛ ma chen.
42005032	N ba wa ɩka n wa bʋɔl a nɩtorsɩ ɛ, n wa naa ɩka n wa bʋɔl a tʋ̃dɛbɛ tʋ̃nbɔ ka ba wa lɩɛb tɩɛr."
42005033	Ka ba lɛ sʋʋr a Yesu, "Ŋmɩnɛ a ɩ ka Jɔɔn poturbo nɩ a Faraseemɩne poturbo ma jɛ̃n kɔ̃ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn, tɩchɛ ka a fʋ̃ʋ poturbo ma tɔ̃ɔ kpal a dib nɩ a nyũfʋ a lɛ a tɔ̃tɔ̃?"
42005034	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Fʋn tʋ̃ɔ maal a bala ban bʋɔl a pɔɔ paalaa jie ka ba jɛ̃n kɔ̃ a pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ na chɛnɛ be a ba sɛ̃ ɔ?
42005035	Tɩchɛ bɩbir kɔ̃ɔ na wa vɩɛ naa ka a pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ yi a ba sɛ̃, a ber ala pɔ 'lɔ ban jɛ̃n nɩ kɔ̃."
42005036	Sʋkpa nyã lɛ wʋ lɔb kʋ ba, "Nɩrɛ maa ŋmaa fɔpaalaa sɛ choo fɔkoraa pɔ ɛ, 'lɔ be ɩ a lɛ a fɔpaalaa na chɩɛraa a fɔkoraa, bʋ̃paalaa nɩ bʋ̃koraa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'mataa ɛ.
42005037	Nɩrɛ maa 'yɔ̃ɔ dãbɩ̃ɩn a dãa wɔkoraa pɔ ɛ, 'lɔ be ɩ a lɛ a dãbɩ̃ɩn na pur naa a wʋɔ ka a dãa kpaar ka a wʋɔ mɩ sɔ̃ɔ.
42005038	Ba ma den dãbɩ̃ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ a dãa wɔpaalaa pɔ.
42005039	Nɩrɛ wa nyũ a dãgaa wʋ maa lɛ bʋɔrɔ a dãbɩ̃ɩn ɛ, wʋ ma 'yɛr ɩka a dãgaa ɩn gar a dãbɩ̃ɩn."
42006001	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ daar, Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo kpɛ̃n tala a puo sãlsɔɔ, ka a wʋ poturbo piel fɔrɔ a bʋ̃bie na ba ŋmɩɛnɛ nɩ a nuur ɔɔrɔ.
42006002	Ka a Farasee bamɩne sʋʋr ba, "Bo lɛ yɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ na ba tara sɔr a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar ɛ?"
42006003	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yaa kar a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ nyɛ a lɛ a David na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ a kɔ̃ na kpɛ ba ɛ?
42006004	Wʋ kpɛ̃n a Nãaŋmɩn yir tɩ de a paanʋ̃ɔ ala ban bin kʋ Nãaŋmɩn na wʋ 'wɔb an ba tara sɔr ɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔrlorbo tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ. Tɩ de amɩne mɩ kʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ."
42006005	Ka a Yesu pãa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Maa Nɩsaal Bie lɛ ɩ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Soro."
42006006	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar ɩ̃sʋɔ, wʋ ben a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir na wʋ wile, ka a daba ɩ̃sʋɔ be be a nũsʋ̃ɔ na kpi.
42006007	A Faraseemɩne nɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe bʋɔrɔ sɔr na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu, lɛ lɛ ba tɔɔ gbʋr kaara wʋ ɩka ba kaa ala ɩ wʋn sãan a baal a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir ɔ.
42006008	Tɩchɛ Yesu bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban tɩɛrɛ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba 'lɔ nũu na kpi, "Ir ara ka nɩrɛ jaa nyɛ fʋ." Ka a daba ir ara.
42006009	Ka a Yesu pãa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N sʋʋr yɩ kaa, bo lɛ sɛɛ ɩka a maal a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar, fʋ maal vɩla bɩɩ fʋ maal dɛɛr? Fʋ kʋ nɩrɛ bɩɩ fʋ faa nɩrɛ, bɩɩ fʋ sɔ̃ɔ bar?"
42006010	Wʋ kãan ba jaa gʋɔr tɩ 'yɛr a daba, "Tur a fʋ nũu." A wʋ tur ka a nũu wʋ jaa sa.
42006011	Tɩchɛ ka a suur kpɛ ba ka ba guoro taa a lɛ ban na ɩ a Yesu.
42006012	A ber ala ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, Yesu don a tɔ̃ɔ ju Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jie, wʋ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn a tɩ̃sɔɔ 'lɔ wʋ jaa.
42006013	A wɛr na wa chaar a bibio, wʋ bʋɔl naa a poturbo ka ba wa a wʋ sɛ̃, ka wʋ ir a ba pɔ pie nɩ ayi bʋɔlɔ ba nɩtʋ̃nsɩ.
42006014	A bala wʋn ir lɛ, Simon wʋn lɛ kʋ yopaalaa Pita, nɩ a wʋ yɛbɛ Andiru, Jemesɩ, Jɔɔn, Filip, Batolomi,
42006015	Matiu, Tomasɩ, Jemesɩ na ɩ Alfayasɩ bidaba, Simon na mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a wʋ wɛr yele,
42006016	Jemesɩ bidaba Judas, nɩ a Judas Isɩkariyot 'lɔ lɛ wa ɩ a gagaraa.
42006017	Yesu tara ban suun ka ba tɩ ara a jie 'lɔ na jɩ̃taa, kaa poturbo yɔɔ be be, ka a nɩyɔɔ mɩ yi Judiya, Jerusalɛm, ka bamɩne mɩ yi a Tire tẽe nɩ a Sidon tẽe na be a man koor.
42006018	Ba wa naa ɩka ba wa chɛl a wʋ 'yɛr tɩ wʋ sãa a ba baalsɩ. Wʋ sãan a bala ba jaa na tara a sɩdɛbɛ.
42006019	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa bʋɔrɔ a Yesu sɩɩrfʋ bojũu kpɛ̃ɔ yire naa a wʋ pɔ sãana a ba jaa baalsɩ.
42006020	Yesu kaara naa a wʋ poturbo tɩ 'yɛr, "Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a yɩn banyãna na ɩ a nɔ̃n dẽme. Yɩn lɛ so a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ.
42006021	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a yɩn a kɔ̃ na kpɛ pʋ̃pãanyã yɩn lɛ na wa tɩɩ. Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a yɩn na kõnõ a pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩn wa laara naa.
42006022	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ yɩ a nɩbɛ na wa 'laar yɩ, na ba oo yɩ bar, tɩ tʋrɔ yɩ na ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yɩ yuor fɩka bʋ̃dɛɛr a maa Nɩsaal Bie jũu.
42006023	A bɩbir nyã wa vɩɛ yɩ chɩlɛ nɩ pʋpɛl, bojũu a yɩ sãyar waa naa na be a saaju. Lɛ lɛ a ba sãakpãmɩne dɔ̃ɔ maal a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ.
42006024	Nɛbier pɔɔn a yɩn na ɩ a tara dẽme, yɩn 'lɔ nyɛn a yɩ 'maalfʋ.
42006025	Nɛbier kpɛ̃n a yɩn na tɩɩ a pʋ̃pãanyã kɔ̃ na kpɛ yɩ naa. Nɛbier kpɛ̃n a yɩn na laara a pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩn lɛ nɩbaal na wa kpɛ a yɩ kõnõ.
42006026	Nɛbier kpɛ̃n a yɩn nɩbɛ jaa na bʋɔlɔ yɩ yo sʋ̃, lɛ lɛ a ba sãakpãmɩne mɩ dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔlɔ a jir 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ a yosʋ̃n.
42006027	"Tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ a yɩn na chɛlɛ a n 'yɛr, yɩ nʋ̃ a yɩ dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃sɩ na yɩ maal vɩla kʋ a bala na 'laar yɩ.
42006028	Yɩ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ, na yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ a bala na gere yɩ.
42006029	Nɩrɛ wa 'ma fʋ tʋkpal pɔ, lɛ lɩɛb a bʋ̃'yen ka wʋ lɛ 'ma, nɩrɛ wa de a fʋ fuu kpɛ̃ɛ ta mɔ̃ɔ wʋ a fuu bile ɛ.
42006030	Nɩrɛ jaa wa sʋɔr fʋ bon de kʋ wʋ, nɩrɛ wa de a fʋ bon taa lɛ wa sʋrɔ wʋ go ɛ.
42006031	A lɛ yɩn bʋɔrɔ ɩka a nɩbɛ ba maal kʋ yɩ, yɩ mɩ maal a lɛ kʋ ba.
42006032	"Ala ɩ yɩ nʋ̃ naa a bala na nʋ̃ yɩ, yobuor lɛ yɩ nyɛ? A yelbetʋ̃nbɔ gba mɩ nʋ̃n a bala na nʋ̃ ba.
42006033	Ala ɩ yɩ maala na vɩla kʋrɔ a bala na maal yɩ a vɩla, yobuor lɛ yɩn nyɛ? A yelbetʋ̃nbɔ gba mɩ ɩrɛ naa a lɛ.
42006034	Ka ala ɩ fʋ pɛ̃ɛn a bala fʋn tɩɛr ɩka ban wa yab fʋ naa, yobuor lɛ yɩn wa nyɛ? A yelbetʋ̃nbɔ ma pɛ̃ɛn a ba taaba tɩɛrɛ ɩka ban wa yab a jaa.
42006035	Tɩchɛ yɩ nʋ̃ a yɩ dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃sɩ na yɩ maal vɩla kʋ ba, yɩ pɛ̃ɛ ba na yɩ taa chɛlɛ ɩka ba lɛ wa yab yɩ ɛ. Ala lɛ a yɩ sãyar na waa, ka yɩ na ɩ a saaju Nãaŋmɩn bibiir, bojũu 'lɔ lɛ maala vɩla kʋrɔ a nɩhayasɩ nɩ putudẽme.
42006036	Yɩ ɩ nɩbibaal dẽme nɩtãa lɛ a yɩ Sãa na ɩ a nɩbibaal sʋɔ.
42006037	"Yɩ ta tɔɔr nɩrɛ 'yɛr ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn mɩ wa tɔɔr a yɩ 'yɛr ɛ. Yɩ ta 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ 'yɛr ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn mɩ ta 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ 'yɛr ɛ. Yɩ vɛ̃ kʋ nɩrɛ ka Nãaŋmɩn mɩ vɛ̃ kʋ yɩ.
42006038	Yɩ de tɩr, Nãaŋmɩn mɩn kʋ yɩ naa, man vɩla tɩ dib 'yɔ̃ɔ tɩ yɛ yɛɛ ka a yaara, an kpaar dɔɔl a yɩ gbɛɛ ju. A bon 'lɔ yɩn man tɩr, 'lɔ mɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na man kʋ yɩ."
42006039	Sʋkpa nyã lɛ a Yesu lɛ lɔb kʋ ba, "Jɔ̃ɔ na tʋ̃ɔn jɔ̃ɔ tɔɔ? Ba jaa ayi kʋ̃ lo bɔɔ pɔ ɛ?
42006040	Nɩrɛ na jãna wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ gar a wʋ wiwile ɛ, tɩ 'lɔ wa jãn baar wʋn tʋ̃ɔ kaara a wʋ wiwile kaar.
42006041	"Ŋmɩnɛ a fʋ kaara a dabile na be a fʋ yɛbɛ nɩbir pɔ, tɩ ba chɛlɛ a dakpɛ̃ɛ na be a fʋ̃ʋ nɩbir pɔ ɛ?
42006042	Bɩɩ Ŋmɩnɛ a ɩ ka fʋ 'yɛr kʋ a fʋ yɛbɛ, n yɛbɛ vɛ̃ ka n ir a a dabile bar a fʋ nɩbir pɔ, tɩ ba ire a dakpɛ̃ɛ na be a fʋ̃ʋ nɩbir pɔ ɛ? Fʋ̃ʋ nɩbɛlɛ nyã, de nie ir a dakpɛ̃ɛ a fʋ nɩbir pɔ bar na fʋ pãa nyɛrɛ tʋ̃ɔ ir a dabile a fʋ yɛbɛ nɩbir pɔ bar.
42006043	"Tɩsʋ̃ ba wɔ̃nɔ̃ bidɛbɛ ɛ, bɩɩ tɩdɛɛr mɩ ba wɔ̃nɔ̃ bisʋ̃n ɛ.
42006044	Tɩɛ jaa a wʋ wɔ̃mɔ̃ lɛ ba ma de bɔ̃ɔn wʋ. Ba maa pɔr kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ gʋtɩɛ ju ɛ, bɩɩ pɔr 'wɔ̃rɔ tamiir tɩɛ ju ɛ.
42006045	Nɩsʋ̃ a yelsʋ̃ ala na be a wʋ pʋɔm lɛ wʋ ma 'yɛrɛ, ka a nɩdɛɛr mɩ ma 'yɛrɛ a yeldɛbɛ ala na be a wʋ pʋɔm. Ala na sɛɛ a pʋɔ lɛ a nɛɛ ma 'yɛrɛ.
42006046	"Ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ bʋɔlɔ ma ɩka Soro, tɩ na yaa turo a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr ɛ?
42006047	Nɩrɛ jaa na wa a n sɛ̃ na wʋ wõ a n 'yɛr tɩ maala, ɩn wiil yɩ naa a lɛ wʋn be.
42006048	Wʋ kaara fɩka nɩrɛ na mɩɛrɛ yir na wʋ tuu a dachin par kparaa bɔɔ tɩ pɔɔn kʋsɩr na mɛ a dachin dɔɔl. Kʋ̃ɔ wa yaar yi jilʋ̃ a yir, ka a kɔ̃sɛbɛ ŋmiere a yir tɩ waa dam ɛ, bojũu ba mɛ wʋn sʋ̃.
42006049	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na wõ a n 'yɛr tɩ na waa maala ɛ, wʋ kaara fɩka nɩrɛ na mɛ yir dɔɔl a tãn mʋɔr ju, waa tuu tɩ mɛ ɛ. A kɔ̃sɛbɛ wa yin ŋme a dachin, ka a dachin wʋ jaa lo ŋmɛr."
42007001	A lɛ a nɩbɛ na wõ a 'yɛrsɩ anyãna a Yesu na 'yɛr kʋ ba baar wʋ chen a Kapenahum.
42007002	Be lɛ a soja nɩdiere gbãgbaa wʋn nʋ̃ yɔɔ jaa bɩɛrɛ ɩrɛ na ŋmaa vʋʋr.
42007003	Soja nɩdiere na wõ a Yesu yele, wʋ tʋ̃n a Juu nɩbɛ nɩdierbe bamɩne ka ba tɩ sʋɔr a Yesu ka wʋ wa sãa a wʋ gbãgbaa.
42007004	Ba wan a Yesu sɛ̃ wa sʋɔr wʋ yãayãabɩlɛ 'yɛrɛ, "A daba nyã sɛɛ naa ɩka fʋ tɩ sʋ̃ʋ wʋ,
42007005	bojũu wʋ nʋ̃n a sɩ nɩbɛ na vɛ̃ ka ba mɛ a sɩ lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie."
42007006	Yesu pɔɔ ba naa ka ba 'mataa chiine tɩ gbʋrɔ a daba yir, ka wʋ tʋ̃ a wʋ barmɩne ka ba tuor 'yɛr a Yesu ɩka. "N Soro, ta bal a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, bojũu n ba sɛɛ ka fʋn wa kpɛ a n yir ɛ.
42007007	Ala lɛ so gba maa mɩ̃ɛ na ba 'la wa a fʋ sɛ̃ ɛ. Tɩchɛ 'yɛr bir tɛɛ an sãan a n gbãgbaa.
42007008	Bojũu maa mɩ̃ɛ tara na nɩbɛrɛ ɩn joro dãbɩ̃ɛ, naa mɩ tara a sojasɩ ka ba mɩ be a n pĩlem. Maa 'yɛr kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩka wʋ, chen wʋ ma chen naa, bɩɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩka wʋ wa, wʋ ma wa naa. N ma 'yɛr kʋ a n gbãgbaa, maal anyã, ka wʋ ma maal."
42007009	A lɛ a Yesu na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ a daba nyã na ba ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ na 'yɛr, ka nɛ'maa wʋ, ka wʋ lɩɛb 'yɛr kʋ a nɩyɔɔ bala. "A Isɩral nɩbɛ pɔ gba, n ba nyɛ a sɔɔfʋ nyã bʋrɔ ɛ."
42007010	Ka a wʋ barmɩne bala wʋn tʋ̃ lɩɛb kpɛ a yir tɩ nyɛ ka a gbãgbaa sa.
42007011	Ala lɛ a wɛr chaar ka Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo 'matãan nɩyɔɔ na turo wʋ ka ba 'mantaa chen a tẽe ban bʋɔlɔ Nain.
42007012	Wʋn wa gbʋr a tẽe dɔ̃dɔr kpɩɛraa ba tuon kũu wa yin na ɩ a pɔɔ bidabʋ̃'yen tɩ wʋ ɩ pɔɔkʋɔr. Ka a tẽe 'lɔ nɩbɛ yɔɔ mɩ pʋɔ wʋ.
42007013	A lɛ a Soro na wa nyɛ a pɔɔ, nɩbaal kpɛ wʋ naa ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a pɔɔ, "Ta kõnõ ɛ."
42007014	Tɩ na wʋ chen tɩ sɩɩr a kũu ban tuo, ka a bala na tuo a ba ara. Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Pɔlbile, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ nɩ ir."
42007015	Ka a kũu vaa ir jɩ̃nɛ tɩ piel na wʋ 'yɛrɛ ka Yesu de wʋ kʋ a ma.
42007016	Dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ̃n ba jaa ka ba pɛɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ nɩ, "Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrkpɛ̃ɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ yi sɩ, Nãaŋmɩn wan ɩka wʋ wa sʋ̃ʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ."
42007017	Ka a Yesu yele ŋme yaar a Judiya paal wʋ jaa nɩ a tẽn ala na gbʋr.
42007018	Jɔɔn poturbo tɩ man a yele anyã a jaa kʋ wʋ, ka wʋ bʋɔl a ba ayi
42007019	na wʋ tʋ̃ ba a Soro sɛ̃ ka ba tɩ sʋʋr wʋ kaa, "Fʋ̃ʋ ɩ a 'lɔ na wa bɩɩ sɩ chɛlɛ nɩyuo?"
42007020	Ka a nɩbɛ bala wa a Yesu sɛ̃ wa 'yɛr, "A Jɔɔn kɔ̃suor lɛ tʋ̃ sɩ a fʋ sɛ̃ ɩka sɩ wa sʋʋr fʋ kaa, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a 'lɔ na wa bɩɩ sɩ chɛlɛ nɩyuo?"
42007021	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ mɩ lɛ Yesu sãa baalsɩ, bala na tara a sɩdɛbɛ na wʋ yuon jɔ̃n nɩbie.
42007022	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a bala a Jɔɔn na tʋ̃, "Yɩ lɩɛb kul tɩ man kʋ a Jɔɔn a lɛ yɩn nyɛ tɩ wõ, jɔ̃n nyɛrɛ naa ka gbɛrsɩ chiine ka kɔ̃kɔ̃n sa, ka wõn wõnõ, ka kũusɩ ir ɩ vʋɛ, ka a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ mɩ ta a nɔ̃n dẽme.
42007023	Pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ a n yele na ba bãr wʋ lɔb ɛ."
42007024	A bala a Jɔɔn na tʋ̃ na wa chen baar, Yesu piel 'yɛrɛ a Jɔɔn 'yɛr kʋrɔ a nɩyɔɔ bala, "Bo lɛ yɩ dɔ̃ɔ kpɛ a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ a kaafʋ jie? A jɩmur a sɛsɛbɛ na dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ bɩɩ?
42007025	Ala ba ɩ lɛ ɛ, bo yɩ chen tɩ nyɛ? Daba na su bʋ̃pɩɛl ɔ? Kai, a bala na suro a bʋ̃sʋ̃n, na ba dire a bʋ̃sʋ̃n nãa yir lɛ ba ma be.
42007026	Tɩchɛ bo lɛ yɩ tɩ nyɛ? Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɔ. Ɔ̃ɔ, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka wʋ gar Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ.
42007027	A anyã yele lɛ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'Ɩn tʋ̃ naa a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ka wʋ de a fʋ nie na wʋ tɩ chɔɔr a fʋ sɔr kʋ fʋ.'
42007028	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka bala pɔɔ na dɔɔ ka a wɛr pɔ ba ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar a Jɔɔn ɛ, tɩchɛ 'lɔ mɩ na ɩ jaa pʋʋr a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ gar wʋ naa."
42007029	Ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa lɔ̃ɔn a lõpodierbe gba na wõ a lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr, ba sɔɔ naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn yele tor naa, na ba sɔɔ ka a Jɔɔn so ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
42007030	Tɩchɛ a Faraseemɩne nɩ a bala na bɔ̃ɔ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ, bala mɩ̃ɛ tɔr naa a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ, bojũu baa sɔɔ ka a Jɔɔn so ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
42007031	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ba boo lɛ ɩn de a dɩna nɩbɛ naa man? Bo lɛ ba nyɛtãan?
42007032	Ba nyɛntãan bibiir na jɩ̃nɛ daa pɔ bʋɔlɔ taa, 'Sɩ pɛɛlɛ naa a laa 'lɩr tɩ yaa sɛɛrɛ bɩ̃nɛ ɛ, na sɩ kõnõ kõyiel tɩ yaa ŋmara nɩbikʋ̃ɔ ɛ.'
42007033	A Jɔɔn kɔ̃suor na wa, waa dire bʋ̃diir ɛ, waa nyuro dãa ɛ, ka yɩ 'yɛr ɩka sɩdɛɛr lɛ wʋ tara.
42007034	Ka a maa Nɩsaal Bie wa na n dire na n nyuro ka yɩ lɛ 'yɛr, 'Wʋ dire na ba gala ɛ, na wʋ nyuro dãa, na wʋ ɩ a lõpodierbe nɩ a tʋ̃dɛtʋ̃nbɔ baraa.'
42007035	Tɩchɛ a yɛ̃ ma wiil a lɛ wʋn tor a wʋ bibiir pɔ."
42007036	A Farasee nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ bʋɔl a Yesu ɩka wʋ wa di bʋ̃diir a wʋ yir, ka wʋ chen a Farasee nɩrɛ 'lɔ yir tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a bʋ̃diir difʋ jie.
42007037	Pɔɔ ben a tẽe pɔ na wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ tʋ̃dɛbɛ, wʋn wa wõ ɩka a Yesu ben a Farasee yir, wʋ den a kãnyũvɩla na sɛɛ pɩ̃rtɔbile na wʋ chiin.
42007038	Wʋ tɩ kpɛ̃n naa na wʋ ara a Yesu gbɛɛ par kõnõ. Wʋ soor a nɩbikʋ̃ɔ 'maan a Yesu gbɛɛ tɩ nyɔɔ a jukɔɔl fɩɛl bar, tɩ mʋʋr a gbɛɛ tɩ kpaar a kãnyũvɩla ala 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu gbɛɛ pɔ.
42007039	Ka a Farasee nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bʋɔl wʋ ka wʋ tɩ dire, na nyɛ a lɛ ka wʋ tɩɛr, "Ala ɩ a daba nyãna ta ɩn Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ wʋn taa bɔ̃ɔn naa a pɔɔ nyãna tɔ sʋɔ na sɩrɛ wʋ, wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ na tʋ̃dɛbɛ."
42007040	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr sɔɔ wʋ, "Simon, n tara na 'yɛr na sʋʋr fʋ." Ka a Simon 'yɛr, "Wiwile, sʋʋr ma."
42007041	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Nɩbɛ ayi kɔ̃ɔ lɛ tɩ pɛ̃ɛ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ libie, ɩ̃sʋɔ pɛ̃ɛn kɔɔr anũu (500) ka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ pɛ̃ɛ lɩjaayi nɩ pie (50).
42007042	A nɩbɛ ayi banyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba tara a libie na yab wʋ ɛ, ka a 'lɔ na so a libie 'yɛr, 'Yɩ ta lɛ yab go ɛ, a sãn baar naa.' Buor sʋɔ lɛ na nʋ̃ wʋ yɔɔ?"
42007043	Ka a Simon 'yɛr, "N tɩɛr ɩka a 'lɔ sãn na waa lɛ." Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ fʋ 'yɛr."
42007044	Yesu lɩɛb tor a pɔɔ tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a Simon, "Fʋ nyɛn a pɔɔ nyãna? Ɩn wa kpɛ a fʋ yir, faa kʋ ma kʋ̃ɔ ɩka n pɛɛ gbɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a pɔɔ pɛɛn a n gbɛɛ nɩ a wʋ nɩbikʋ̃ɔ tɩ de a wʋ jukɔɔl fɩɛl bar.
42007045	Faa sʋʋr ma kpɩ̃ɛn ɛ, tɩchɛ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa ɩn wa kpɛ a pɔɔ nyã ba bar ma kpɩ̃ɛn sʋʋrfʋ ɛ.
42007046	Faa pur kãa 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a ju pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ a pɔɔ kpaar a kãnyũvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a gbɛɛ pɔ.
42007047	A lɛ jũu n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ fʋ ɩka a wʋ tʋ̃dɛbɛ ala a jaa vɛ̃n kʋ wʋ, bojũu a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ waa naa. Tɩchɛ a 'lɔ Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ jaa pʋʋr kʋ a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ mɩ ɩn jaa pʋʋr."
42007048	A Yesu pãa 'yɛr kʋ a pɔɔ, "A fʋ yeldɛbɛ vɛ̃n bar."
42007049	Ka a bala na lɔ̃ɔ jɛ̃n wʋ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "An lɛ anyã, na wʋ mɩ ma vɛ̃ nɩrɛ yeldɛɛr bar?"
42007050	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a pɔɔ, "A fʋ sɔɔfʋ faa fʋ naa, chiine nɩ nyã'maar."
42008001	A anyãna puor, Yesu yɔn a tẽbɛrɛ nɩ a tẽbil 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr kʋrɔ ba ka a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nsɩ Pie nɩ Ayi pʋɔ wʋ.
42008002	Ka a pɔbɔ bamɩne mɩ pʋɔ wʋ, bala lɛ wʋ dɔ̃ɔ dii a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi na wʋ sãa a ba baalsɩ, ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ ba bʋɔlɔ Mɛɛr na yi a Magdala 'lɔ lɛ wʋ dii a sɩdɛbɛ ayopõi ka a yi,
42008003	Joana lɛ a ɩ̃sʋɔ na ɩ a Kuja na kaara a Hɛrɔd yir pɔɔ, Susana lɛ a ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩ a pɔbɔ yɔɔ bamɩne. Banyãna lɛ de a ba bomo sʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo.
