42008004	Nɩyɔɔ yin tẽn tẽn waara a Yesu sɛ̃, a nɩyɔɔ banyãna na wa duo, sʋkpa nyã lɛ wʋ lɔb kʋ ba,
42008005	"Kʋɔraa lɛ yin wʋ bʋ̃bʋrɔ bʋrfʋ jie. Wʋ tɩ yaara naa yʋɔrɔ nɩ ka amɩne tɩ lo sɔr pɔ, ka ba nɛ nɛb ka lubil wa tuur di.
42008006	Ka amɩne mɩ tɩ lo kʋsɩr pãn ju naa bul tɩ kpi bojũu tãn ba be be ɛ.
42008007	Ka amɩne mɩ lo gʋʋr pɔ 'mataa bul ka a gʋʋr nʋ̃ɔ fɩ̃ɩn ba.
42008008	Tɩchɛ ka amɩne mɩ lo a kɔjɔ̃ pɔ bul dɔɔ jur kɔɔkɔɔr naa gar a lɛ wʋn bʋr." Yesu na wa 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ baar, wʋ 'yɛr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, "Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara tuor wõnõ nɩ wʋ chɛlɛ."
42008009	Ka a wʋ poturbo sʋʋr wʋ a sʋkpa nyã par.
42008010	A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn 'lɔ, n vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ yelsɔɔlsɩ, tɩchɛ a bala na chɛ, sʋkpar lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ ba, 'Ba ma kaa naa tɩ maa nyɛ ɛ, na ba ma wõnõ tɩ ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ.'
42008011	"A sʋkpa par nɩ nyã. Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr lɛ ɩ a bʋ̃bie.
42008012	A ala na lo a sɔr pɔ ɩn a bala na wõ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr, tɩchɛ ka a tɩɩ wa ir naa a ba nyãa pɔ, ka ba ta sɔɔ de nyɛ faafʋ ɛ.
42008013	Ala mɩ na lo a kʋsɩr pãn ju ɩn a bala na wõ a 'yɛr den pʋpɛl, tɩchɛ baa tara nyɩbɛ ɛ. Ba sɔɔn ara bɩ̃lãa tɩchɛ bɛɛr kaa wa wa ba ma lo naa.
42008014	A bʋ̃bie ala na lo a gʋʋr pɔ ɩn a bala na wõ a 'yɛr, tɩchɛ ka a ɩ̃gãn nyã vɔlaa nɩ bʋ̃tarsɩ nɩ a bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ fɩ̃ɩn ba ka baa tʋ̃ɔ dɔɔ bie ɛ.
42008015	Tɩchɛ a bʋ̃bie ala na lo a kɔjɔ̃ pɔ, ɩn a bala na wõ a 'yɛr na ba sɔɔ den nyãa ara nɩ pʋpɛl, ka a kãnyir vɛ̃ ka ba dɔɔ jur.
42008016	"Nɩrɛ jaa maa chʋm fɩ̃tɩn de laa kpa pɔɔ ɛ, bɩɩ de su gado pĩlem ɛ. Tɩchɛ wʋ ma den dɔɔl a dɔɔlfʋ jie ka a bala na kpɩɛrɛ nyɛ a chãa.
42008017	Bojũu bon jaa ba be be na sɔɔl ka ba kʋ̃ nyɛ wʋ ɛ, bɩɩ bon jaa ba be be sɔɔl ka ba kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔn ɛ, bɩɩ kʋ̃ yi chãa pɔ ɛ.
42008018	A lɛ jũu, yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃ a lɛ yɩn chɛlɛ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bɔ̃ɔ a par Nãaŋmɩn na lɛ kʋ wʋn dɔɔl, nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn na den a bɩ̃lãa 'lɔ wʋn tɩɛr ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔn a par."
42008019	Yesu ma nɩ a wʋ yɛɛr wan ɩka ba wa nyɛ wʋ, tɩchɛ a nɩyɔɔ jũu ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ɛ.
42008020	Ka nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr wʋ, "A fʋ ma nɩ a fʋ yɛɛr lɛ be a yõo bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba nyɛ fʋ."
42008021	A Yesu 'yɛr, "N ma nɩ a n yɛɛr lɛ a bala na wõ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr na ba turo."
42008022	Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "Yɩ ɩ a sɩ gɔ̃ɔ a kasɛn a manyal gɔ̃ɔn." Be lɛ ba kpɛ a gboro na ba gɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
42008023	Ban gɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ tɩ wʋ gã gur. Ka a kɔ̃sɛkpɛ̃ɛ ire a man pɔ ka a kʋ̃ɔ ɔɔrɔ kpɩɛrɛ a gboro pɔ, ka ba ɩrɛ na mʋr.
42008024	Ka a poturbo tɩ sɩ̃ɩ wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Kpãkpãana, a kʋ̃ɔ na di sɩ naa." Ka a Yesu ir tãn a sɛsɛbɛ nɩ a kʋ̃ɔ na ɔɔrɔ, ka a sɛsɛbɛ ŋmaa vʋʋr ka a kʋ̃ɔ mɩ lo jaa jomm....
42008025	Tɩ pãa sʋʋr a wʋ poturbo, "Nyɩnɛ a yɩ sɔɔfʋ be?" Ka ba mɩ de dãbɩ̃ɛ sʋrɔ nɩ taa, "Nɩ an lɛ anyã, na 'yɛr ka a sɛsɛbɛ nɩ kʋ̃ɔ tu a wʋ nɛɛ?"
42008026	Ba yin a Galilee gɔ̃ɔn na ba gɔ̃ɔ a Gerasenɩ gɔ̃ɔn.
42008027	Yesu na wa yire a gogoro ju wʋ tuor daba na tara sɩdɛbɛ na wʋ gele yi a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ. Bojũu a kor wʋn yi a yir na wʋ maa su fuu ɛ, tɩ na wʋ gãna a yar par.
42008028	Wʋn wa nyɛ a Yesu wʋ ŋmen chɛlma tɩ lo a Yesu niem na wʋ tãna 'yɛrɛ nɩ, "Bo lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ ka a n sɛ̃, a fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ a saaju Nãaŋmɩn Bie? N sʋɔrɔ fʋ naa, ta ge ma ɛ."
42008029	Bojũu Yesu dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a sɩdɛɛr ɩka wʋ yi a daba 'yɔ̃ɔ. Gbɛɛ yɔɔ jaa lɛ a ma ir a daba ka ba ma gbar a nuur nɩ a gbɛɛ nɩ bɔ̃jɔrsɩ kaara wʋ, tɩ wʋ ma kar a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ bar ka a sɩdɛɛr ma dii wʋ bar be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ wʋ yõ.
42008030	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "A fʋ yuor lɛ di bo?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Nɩyɔɔ." Bojũu sɩdɛyɔɔ lɛ kpɛ wʋ.
42008031	Ka a sɩdɛbɛ sʋɔrɔ a Yesu ɩka wʋ ta dii ba 'yɔ̃ɔ be a bɔɔ fulom 'lɔ pɔ ɛ.
42008032	Doyɔɔ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ara be a tɔ̃ɔ kõkoor dire, ka a sɩdɛbɛ sʋɔr a Yesu ɩka wʋ sɔɔ ka ba yi tɩ kpɛ a dor ala pɔ, ka wʋ sɔɔ kʋ ba sɔr.
42008033	A sɩdɛbɛ yin a daba pɔ tɩ kpɛ a dor pɔ, ka a tĩgbil suu tɩ kpɛ a man kʋ̃ɔ pɔ tɩ gbʋ̃m kpi kpi.
42008034	A bala na kaara a dor na wa nyɛ a lɛ na ɩ, ba jon kul a tẽe pɔ, nɩ a tẽbil ala na gbʋr tɩ 'yɛr a lɛ na ɩ.
42008035	Ka a nɩbɛ yi chen ɩka ba tɩ kaa a lɛ na ɩ. Ba chen a Yesu sɛ̃ tɩ nyɛ a dagẽgelaa a sɩdɛbɛ na yi tɩ chɛ bar ka wʋ chɩ na wʋ su a fuu jɩ̃nɛ a Yesu gbɛɛ par, ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba.
42008036	A nɩbɛ bala na dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ a lɛ an ɩ ka a gẽgelaa sa pãa mana kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ.
42008037	Ka a Gerasenɩ paal nɩbɛ ba jaa sʋɔrɔ a Yesu ɩka wʋ yi a be, bojũu dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba naa. Lɛ lɛ wʋ kpɛ a gboro yi a be chen.
42008038	Ka a daba 'lɔ pɔ a sɩdɛbɛ na yi sʋɔr a Yesu ɩka ba 'mataa chen, tɩchɛ a Yesu lɩɛb wʋ bar tɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ,
42008039	"Lɩɛb kul a fʋ yir tɩ man a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ kʋ fʋ." Lɛ lɛ ka a daba kul a tẽe pɔ tɩ mana kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ a lɛ a Yesu na ɩ kʋ wʋ.
42008040	Yesu na wa lɩɛb wa, a nɩyɔɔ tuor de wʋ, bojũu ba dɔ̃ɔ chɛlɛ wʋ.
42008041	Ka daba ban bʋɔlɔ Jairusɩ na ɩ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir nɩdier, wa gbur dumo a Yesu niem sʋɔrɔ wʋ yãayãabɩlɛ ɩka wʋ wa a wʋ yir,
42008042	bojũu a wʋ bipɔɔ bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ na nyɛ yuom pie nɩ ayi lɛ kpire. Yesu na de a sɔr chiine ka a nɩyɔɔ mɩl pɔɔ wʋ.
42008043	Ka pɔɔ mɩ be be na lo sɩɛ suoro faara yuom pie nɩ ayi, nɩrɛ jaa ba tʋ̃ɔ wʋ sãa ɛ.
42008044	A wʋ turo a puor tɩ sɩɩr a Yesu fuu nɛɛ ka a jɩ̃ɩ ŋmaa ajienaa.
42008045	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr, "An lɛ sɩɩr ma?" Ka ba jaa chiir ɩka baa sɩɩr wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a Pita 'yɛr, "N Soro, a nɩbɛ waa naa na dara taa tɩɛr fʋ."
42008046	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ sɩɩr ma na wʋ sa ka n bɔ̃ɔn."
42008047	A pɔɔ na wa nyɛ ka ɩ wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ sɔɔl ɛ, wʋ mɩrɛ naa wa lo gã a Yesu niem. A nɩyɔɔ bala niem tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr a lɛ jũu wʋn sɩɩr wʋ na wʋ sa ajienaa.
42008048	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N bipɔɔ, a fʋ sɔɔfʋ sa fʋ naa, kulo nɩ nyã'maar."
42008049	Yesu na chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ, nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ yin a lɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩdier Jairusɩ yir wa 'yɛrɛ, "A fʋ bipɔɔ kpi naa ta lɛ fɩrɛ a wiwile go ɛ."
42008050	Yesu na wõ a lɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Jairusɩ, "Ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Sɔɔ ma dɛ. Wʋn sa naa."
42008051	Wʋn wa ta a Jairusɩ yir waa sɔɔ ka nɩyuo kpɛ be ɛ, tɩ tara Pita, Jɔɔn nɩ Jemesɩ nɩ a bi sãa nɩ a ma kpɛ̃n.
42008052	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na kõnõ ŋmiere a chɛlsɩ, Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bar a kõn waa kpi ɛ, wʋ gur naa."
42008053	Ka ba laara wʋ ban bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a bie kpi naa.
42008054	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu nyɔɔ a bie nũu tɩ 'yɛr, "N bie, ir."
42008055	Ka wʋ sɩɛ lɩɛb wa kpɛ ka wʋ vaa ir. Ka a Yesu pãa 'yɛr, yɩ kʋ wʋ bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ di.
42008056	Ka a sãa naa ma nyɔɔ nɛɛ, tɩchɛ ka a Yesu kpãkpãan ba ɩka ba taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa a lɛ na ɩ ɛ.
42009001	Yesu na wa bʋɔl a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nsɩ pie nɩ ayi lɔ̃ɔ taa, wʋ kʋ ban kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ tʋ̃ɔfʋ ka ban diin sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi tɩ sãa baalsɩ.
42009002	Wʋ tʋ̃ ba naa ka ba chen tɩ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr tɩ sãa baal.
42009003	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ taa tara bon jaa chiine ɛ. Yɩ ta de dãgbal ɛ, bɩɩ wʋɔ ɛ, bɩɩ bʋ̃diir ɛ, bɩɩ libie ɛ, bɩɩ de fuusɩ ayi ɛ.
42009004	Yir jaa pɔ yɩn tɩ kpɛ, yɩ jɩ̃nɛ a be tɩ tãn a daar 'lɔ yɩn na yi a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ.
42009005	Ala ɩ nɩbɛ ba wa de yɩ ɛ, yɩ yi a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ, tɩ yɩn wa yire yɩ pĩ pĩ a yɩ gbɛɛ tã-uul ka a di a ba dãasɩɛ."
42009006	Be lɛ ba yi lʋɔrɔ a tẽn tẽn 'yɛrɛ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã sãa na nɩ a nɩbɛ baalsɩ a jie wʋ jaa.
42009007	A Nãa Hɛrɔd na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ na ɩrɛ, ka tɩɛr nyɔɔ wʋ, bojũu bamɩne 'yɛrɛ naa ɩka Jɔɔn lɛ tɔ̃ɔ ir ɩ vʋr.
42009008	Ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛrɛ ɩka a Elaija lɛ tɔ̃ɔ yi, ka bamɩne mɩ chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ tɔ̃ɔ ir ɩ vʋr.
42009009	Tɩchɛ ka a Hɛrɔd 'yɛr, "N ŋmaan Jɔɔn ju, tɩ an 'yɛr lɛ a nyã ɩn wõnõ?" Na wʋ mʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ nyɛ a Yesu.
42009010	A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ lɩɛb wa na ba wa man kʋ a Yesu a lɛ ban tʋ̃. Ka wʋ pãa tara a bala tɛɛ ka ba 'mataa chen a tẽe ban bʋɔlɔ Betɩsaida.
42009011	Tɩchɛ ka a nɩyɔɔ chɛnɛ bɔ̃ɔn na ba bɩɛr chen a jie. Wʋ de ba naa na wʋ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, tɩ sãa a bala na bʋɔrɔ a sãafʋ.
42009012	Mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa mʋrɔ, a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ pie nɩ ayi tɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wɛl a nɩbɛ bar a ba chen a tẽbil anyã nɩ a por anyã na gbʋr na ba tɩ bɔ gaa jie nɩ bʋ̃diir di bojũu a ka ɩn mɔgɔ̃ɔ."
42009013	Ka wʋ 'yɛr sɔɔ ba, "Yɩn lɛ na kʋ ba bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ ka ba di." Ka ba 'yɛr, "Paanʋ̃ɔsɩ anũu nɩ jɩ̃bie ayi tɛɛ lɛ sɩ tara, ka a ba ɩ sɩ chen tɩ da bʋ̃diir wa kʋ a nɩyɔɔ ba nyãna ɛ?"
42009014	A nɩyɔɔ bala, dɔɔr tɛɛ ɩn tur anũu (5,000). Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo, "Yɩ ŋma a nɩbɛ ka ba jɩ̃nɛ jɩ̃nɛ gbulsɩ lɩjaayi nɩ pie pie."
42009015	A poturbo ɩn a lɛ ka nɩrɛ jaa jɛ̃ tẽe.
42009016	Yesu den a paanʋ̃ɔsɩ a nũu nɩ a jɩ̃mɛ ayi ala dʋl kaa saaju tɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, tɩ na wʋ ŋma ŋma, de kʋ a poturbo ɩka ba de põ a nɩbɛ.
42009017	Ba jaa din tɩɩ, ka a poturbo wob a bʋ̃ŋmaar ala na chɛ sɛɛ pɛr pie nɩ ayi.
42009018	Daar kɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Yesu tɛɛ wa sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka wʋ poturbo be be ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "An lɛ a nɩbɛ 'yɛrɛ ɩka n ɩ naa?"
42009019	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Bamɩne 'yɛr ɩka fʋ ɩn a Jɔɔn 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr ɩka Elaija lɛ, ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ lɩɛb wa."
42009020	Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Tɩchɛ yɩn mɩ, an lɛ yɩ 'yɛr ɩka n ɩ naa?" Ka a Pita 'yɛr, "Fʋ ɩ naa a Nɩ-iraa yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃."
42009021	Ka a Yesu kpãkpãan ba ɩka ba taa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ.
42009022	Tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, "A maa Nɩsaal Bie na din dɔɔyɛ yɔɔ ka a nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe tɔr ma bar, ka ba kʋ ma, ka a ber ata daar ka n ir ɩ vʋr."
42009023	Be lɛ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba jaa, "Ala ɩ nɩrɛ na turo ma naa, wʋ 'laar a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩ tuo a wʋ daa turo nɩ ma.
42009024	Bojũu nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ faa a wʋ nyɛvʋr a wʋ nyɛvʋr na bɔr naa, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na lɔb a wʋ nyɛvʋr bar a maa jũu na faa wʋ naa.
42009025	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ tara naa a wɛr wʋ jaa bonsɩ tɩ bɔr bɩɩ ka a wʋ sɩɛ wɛ, bo tɔ̃nɔ̃ wʋ nyɛ?
42009026	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ nyɛ naa maa nɩ a n 'yɛr ka a ɩ vĩ yele a wʋ sɛ̃, a maa Nɩsaal Bie mɩ na kaa naa nɩnyɩnɛ ka wʋ ɩ vĩ sʋɔ maa wa lɩɛb waara nɩ a n tɩɩr nɩ a Sãa tɩɩr nɩ a malaka chɛchɛ bala.
42009027	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a yɩ bamɩne gba ara naa kana kʋ̃ kpi ɛ, tɩ na ban nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ."
42009028	Yesu na 'yɛr a 'yɛrbie anyãna baar a maal ber aniin tɩ wʋ tara Pita, Jɔɔn nɩ Jemesɩ don a tɔ̃ɔ ju Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jie.
42009029	Wʋn tɩ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn ka a nie lɩɛb, ka a fuu pɛl nyɩlɛ bũu 'lɩraa kaar.
42009030	Ka a dɔɔr ayi, Mosesɩ nɩ Elaija wa naa a wʋ sɛ̃.
42009031	Ba wa yin naa a saaju tɩɩr 'yɛrɛ nɩ a Yesu. Ba 'mantaa 'yɛrɛ a kũu a Yesu na tɩ kpi a Jerusalɛm 'yɛr.
42009032	Gʋ̃ɔ kpɛ̃n a Pita nɩ a wʋ taaba, tɩchɛ ban wa jɔɔ ir ba nyɛn a wʋ tɩɩr nɩ a dɔɔr ayi bala a ba ara a wʋ sɛ̃.
42009033	A dɔɔr bala na lɩɛb chiine ka Pita 'yɛr, "N Soro, a sɛɛn ka sɩn kpɩɛrɛ a ka. Bar a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ sɛɛr ata, fʋ̃ʋ so ɩ̃sʋɔ, Mosesɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ Elaija mɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ." Waa bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ ɛ.
42009034	Wʋn chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ a julõjuur wa pɔɔn ba jaa ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a Pita, Jɔɔn nɩ Jemesɩ.
42009035	Ka a kɔkɔr yi be a julõjuur pɔ 'yɛrɛ, "Nyã lɛ ɩ a n Bie ɩn ir, yɩ chɛlɛ a wʋ 'yɛr."
42009036	A kɔkɔr na wa 'yɛr baar, ba nyɛn a Yesu tɛɛ na ara. Ka a poturbo ba 'la man kʋ nɩrɛ a lɛ ban nyɛ ɛ.
42009037	A wɛr na wa chaar, ba yin a tɔ̃ɔ ju suu, a nɩyɔɔ wa lɔ̃ɔ a wʋ sɛ̃.
42009038	Ka a daba bʋɔl be a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ, "Wiwile, n sʋɔrɔ fʋ naa, kaa a n bidaba, 'lɔ tɛɛ lɛ ɩ a n bie.
42009039	Sɩɛ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ tara wʋ, ma ire wʋ ba gala ɛ. Wʋ maa ŋmen a chɛlma tɩ tãanaa tɩ furo a natafuul a nɛɛ pɔ. Wʋ maa bara wʋ ɛ, na wʋ bʋɔrɔ a wʋ sɔ̃ɔfʋ.
42009040	N sʋɔr a fʋ poturbo ɩka ba dii a sɩɛ nyã bar tɩchɛ baa tʋ̃ɔ ɛ."
42009041	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩn babãma dẽme na ba tara sɔɔfʋ ɛ, n be a yɩ sɛ̃ naa tara yɩ nɩ kãnyir tɩ tãn dabor?" Tɩ 'yɛr a daba, "Tɔɔ a bie wa kʋ ma!"
42009042	A bie na chɛnɛ waara ka a sɩdɛɛr ir a bie tãa lɔb a tẽe, tɩchɛ ka a a Yesu tãn a sɩdɛɛr na wʋ sãa a bie de kʋ a sãa.
42009043	Nɩbɛ ba jaa nɛ'maa naa ban nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ. A nɩbɛ na chɛnɛ kpire a lɛ a Yesu na ɩ, tɩ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo,
42009044	"Yɩ chɛlɛ a lɛ ɩn 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ban gar naa maa Nɩsaal Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɩbɛ nuur pɔ."
42009045	Tɩchɛ baa bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna wʋn 'yɛr par ɛ, a lii ba naa, ka ba bɔ̃ɔ faa, tɩ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ba 'la sʋʋr wʋ ɛ.
42009046	Nɛchɩrɛ ir naa a Yesu poturbo pɔ ɩka a ba buor sʋɔ lɛ na ɩ a ba kpɛ̃ɛ.
42009047	Yesu na bɔ̃ɔ a ba tɩɛr, wʋ tɔɔn bibile wa lan a wʋ lõboor.
42009048	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩrɛ jaa na de a bibile nyãna a maa jũu maa lɛ wʋ de. Nɩrɛ jaa mɩ na de ma wʋ mɩ den a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma. Bojũu nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ɩ a yɩ jaa bile, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar yɩ jaa."
42009049	Ka a Jɔɔn 'yɛr, "N Soro, sɩ nyɛn nɩrɛ na de a fʋ yuor dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire, ka sɩ 'yɛr wʋ ɩka wʋ ta ɩrɛ a lɛ ɛ, bojũu waa ɩ a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ."
42009050	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩ ta ŋmaa wʋ sɔr ɛ, bojũu nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba kpɛrɛ yɩ ɛ, wʋ pʋɔ yɩ naa."
42009051	Lɛ a sɔ̃ɔ na wa gbʋrɔ ka Yesu na lɩɛb do a saaju, wʋ ŋmen nyãa a Jerusalɛm chenfʋ.
42009052	Wʋ den nie tʋ̃ nɩbɛ ka ba de nie chen a Samariya tẽbile ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, na ban tɩ chɔɔr a jie bar wʋ.
42009053	Tɩchɛ a tẽe 'lɔ nɩbɛ ba sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ, bojũu Jerusalɛm lɛ wʋ chiine.
42009054	Ka a wʋ poturbo Jemesɩ nɩ Jɔɔn na wa nyɛ a lɛ, ka ba sʋʋr a Yesu, "Sɩ Soro, fʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka sɩ bʋɔl bũu ka ayi saaju suu wa di ba bɩɩ?"
42009055	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu lɩɛb tãn ba ɩka ba ta ɩ a lɛ ɛ.
42009056	Tɩ na ba chen tẽyuo pɔ.
42009057	A sɔr ban chɛnɛ de chiine ka daba ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Jie jaa fʋn chiine ɩn turo fʋ naa!"
42009058	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Mɔbaar tara naa bɔɔr ka a lubil mɩ tara choor, tɩchɛ maa Nɩsaal Bie ba tara jie na bin a n ju ɛ."
42009059	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba ɩ̃sʋɔ, "Turo ma." Tɩchɛ ka a daba 'yɛr, "N Soro, bar ma sɔr ka n kul tɩ ũu a n sãa baar."
42009060	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a daba, "Bar ka a kũn ũno ba mɩ̃ɛ kũn tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ, chen tɩ mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr."
42009061	Ka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr, "N Soro, ɩn turo fʋ naa tɩ bar ma sɔr ka n kul tɩ 'yɛr a n yir dẽme."
42009062	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ na nyɔɔ niin kuur tɩ lɩɛb kaara a puor ba sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ."
42010001	A nyã puor Yesu lɛ ir naa nɩbɛ lɩjaata nɩ pie nɩ ayi (72) bamɩne go, na wʋ tʋ̃ ba ayir yir ka ba de nie chen a tẽn nɩ a jiir ala a jaa wʋn na yɔ.
42010002	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A puo bɛr ma naa, tɩchɛ ka a bala na ŋmara ba waa ɛ, a lɛ jũu yɩ sʋɔr a puo sɔɔ ka wʋ waan tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a puo pɔ.
42010003	Yɩ chen, yɩ kaara na fɩka piir ɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃ ka yɩn tɩ kpɛ gbõgborosɩ pɔ.
42010004	Yɩ taa de libie ɛ, bɩɩ wʋɔ ɛ, bɩɩ na fɔɔr ɛ, na yɩ puor nɩrɛ taa wa jaa a sɔr pɔ ɛ.
42010005	"Yir jaa pɔ yɩn wa kpɛ, yɩ de nie 'yɛr, 'Nyã'maar wʋ be a yir nyã pɔ.'
42010006	Ala ɩ nyã'maar sʋɔ ben a yir pɔ, a yɩ nyã'maar na be naa a wʋ sɛ̃, ala ba ɩ lɛ ɛ, an lɩɛb wa a yɩ sɛ̃.
42010007	Yɩ jɩ̃nɛ a yir nyɩnɛ pɔ dire na yɩ nyuro bon jaa ban wa kʋ yɩ, tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ sãyar sɛɛn wʋ naa. Yɩ taa lʋɔrɔ yie yʋɔrɔ nɩ ɛ.
42010008	Tẽe jaa pɔ yɩn wa kpɛ, ka ba de yɩ, yɩ dire bon jaa ban kʋ yɩ.
42010009	Yɩ sãana a baalsɩ bala na be be tɩ na yɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'A Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ gbʋr yɩ naa.'
42010010	Tɩchɛ tẽe jaa pɔ yɩn wa kpɛ, ka baa de yɩ ɛ, yɩ yi de a tẽe sãlsɔɔ tɩ 'yɛr,
42010011	'A yɩ tẽe tã-uul gba na mar a sɩ gbɛɛ, sɩ kpoor 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ. Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a nyãna ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ gbʋr naa.'
42010012	N 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ bɩbir, Sodom na sa naa a tẽe 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
42010013	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn Korajin dẽme sɛ̃, nɛbier mɩ ben a yɩn Betɩsaida dẽme mɩ sɛ̃. A nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala ɩn tʋ̃ a yɩ jie, ala ɩ a mɩ ta tʋ̃n a lɛ a Tire nɩ Sidon tẽe pɔ, ban taa sun bʋ̃jarsɩ jɛ̃n tãpɩɛl pɔ lɩɛb ba tɩɛr.
42010014	Tɩchɛ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar, a Tire nɩ a Sidon na sa yɩ naa.
42010015	A yɩn Kapenahum dẽme, ban 'mɔɔ yɩn don saaju bɩɩ? Kai, ban suun yɩ naa kpĩisɩ tẽe.
42010016	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na chɛlɛ a yɩn na ɩ a n poturbo na chɛl naa a n 'yɛr, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tɔr yɩ mɩ tɔr ma naa. Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tɔr ma mɩ tɔr naa a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma."
42010017	A nɩbɛ lɩjaata nɩ pie nɩ ayi bala wʋn tʋ̃ lɩɛb wa a wʋ sɛ̃ chɩlɛ 'yɛrɛ, "Sɩ Soro, a fʋ yuor jũu a sɩdɛbɛ tu naa a sɩ nɛɛ na be yire a nɩbɛ pɔ."
42010018	Ka Yesu 'yɛr sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, "N nyɛn Satan na yi saaju lo fɩka saa na nyɩɩr.
42010019	N kʋ yɩn kpɛ̃ɔ ka yɩn nɛɛrɛ waba nɩ lɔ̃n na yɩ tʋ̃ɔ a yɩ dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃ Satan, bon jaa kʋ̃ ɩ yɩ ɛ.
42010020	Yɩ ta chɩlɛ a sɩdɛbɛ na tu a yɩ nɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ chɩlɛ a yɩ yuor sɛb bin be a saaju."
42010021	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a Yesu ka wʋ 'yɛr, "N dãn a fʋ̃ʋ n Sãa na ɩ a saaju nɩ a tẽe Soro, bojũu fʋ̃ʋ lɛ sɔɔl a yele anyãna bar ka a bala na ɩ a yɛ̃ dẽme nɩ a bala na jãn ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ na fʋ de wiil kʋ bibiir. Ɔ̃ɔ, n Sãa lɛ lɛ nʋ̃mɔ̃ fʋ ka fʋ maal.
42010022	Maa lɛ a n Sãa kʋ a yele a jaa, nɩrɛ jaa ba bɔ̃ɔ a Bie ka a Sãa ba lɛ ɛ. Nɩrɛ jaa mɩ ba bɔ̃ɔ a Sãa ka a Bie ba lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala a maa Nãaŋmɩn Bie na ir, na wiil naa a sãa kʋ ba. Ka ba bɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na be."
42010023	Tɩ pãa lɩɛb 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo tɛɛ, "Pʋpɛl dẽme lɛ a bala nɩbir na nyɛ a anyã yɩn nyɛ.
42010024	Bojũu n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ nɩ a nãmɩne dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba nyɛ a anyã yɩn nyɛ, tɩ ba nyɛ ɛ, na ba ta wõ a anyã yɩn wõ tɩ ba wõ ɛ."
42010025	Nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na bɔ̃ɔ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ bɛɛr a Yesu kaa na wʋ ir sʋʋr, "Wiwile, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ɩn ɩ naa nyɛ nyɛvʋr kpo kpo?"
42010026	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Bo ba sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ bin? Ŋmɩnɛ fʋ ma kar?"
42010027	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "Nʋ̃ a fʋ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a fʋ nyãa wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ nyɛvʋr wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ kpɛ̃ɔ wʋ jaa, nɩ a fʋ tɩɛr wʋ jaa. Na fʋ nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ nɩtãa a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ."
42010028	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr, "Fʋ 'yɛr vɩla, tɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ, fʋn ben be kpo kpo."
42010029	Tɩchɛ wʋn ba ɩrɛ a lɛ ɛ, tɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ sɔɔl a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ bar jũu, wʋ sʋʋr naa Yesu, "Nɩbuor lɛ ɩ a n tɔ sʋɔ?"
42010030	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Daba kɔ̃ɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ yi Jerusalɛm chiine Jeriko ka a nãnyisɩ tɩ var wʋ be a sɔr pɔ. Ba yaar naa fuusɩ tɩ ŋme ŋme wʋ, ka wʋ vɔɔ chɛ bɩ̃lãa naa kpi, ka ba bar wʋ tɩ chen.
42010031	A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrloro ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ de a sɔr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, wʋn tɩ nyɛ a daba, wʋ gõl bar tɩ chen.
42010032	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn Puorfʋ yir tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ waara wa nyɛ, na wʋ mɩ gõl tu jiyuo chen.
42010033	Tɩchɛ ka a nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na ɩ a Samariya nɩrɛ mɩ tu a sɔr 'lɔ a daba na gã, wʋn wa nyɛ wʋ, nɩbaal kpɛ wʋ naa.
42010034	Ka wʋ tɔɔ ta a daba pʋr dãa pɛɛn a natɩɛ bar, tɩ maal kãa fɔ, tɩ de fɔbaa lũ pɔɔ. Na wʋ 'mɔɔ a daba dɔɔl a wʋ bʋ̃ɔ ju chiin a sãanba gaa jie tɩ gãn.
42010035	Wɛr na wa chaar, wʋ den a kpãna libikue ayi kʋ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kaara a sãanba tɩ 'yɛr, 'Kaara wʋ, maa wa lɩɛb gɔr, ala ba wa ta ɛ, ɩn lɛ yab kʋ fʋ.' "
42010036	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr a daba, "A nɩbɛ ata banyãna, buor sʋɔ lɛ ɩ a daba nyã, a nãnyisɩ na ŋme tɔ sʋɔ?"
42010037	A wʋ 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kaa a wʋ nɩbaal." Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Mɩ chen tɩ maal a lɛ nɛ."
42010038	Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo na chiine ba vɩɛn kpɛ tẽbile kɔ̃ɔ pɔ, ka pɔɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Mata ka wʋ de ba na ir ba sãan.
42010039	A Mata tara na yɛbɛ ban bʋɔlɔ Mɛɛr, ka 'lɔ jɩ̃nɛ a Soro gbɛɛ par chɛlɛ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ.
42010040	Tɩchɛ ka a Mata wʋ yõ sõsoro nɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃, na wʋ wa tɔɔ ta a Yesu sɛ̃ 'yɛr, "N Soro, a ba bã fʋ a n yɛbɛ na bar a tʋ̃mɔ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ ma ka n sõsoro nɩ ɛ? 'Yɛr wʋ ka wʋ ir wa sʋ̃ʋ ma."
42010041	Ka a Soro 'yɛr, "Mata, Mata fʋ fɩrɛ na fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ka suur kʋrɔ fʋ.
42010042	Tɩchɛ yelbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ fɛr, Mɛɛr ir naa a bʋ̃sʋ̃ nɩrɛ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ faa wʋ yin a wʋ sɛ̃ ɛ."
42011001	Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ Yesu ben a jie kɔ̃ɔ na wʋ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn, wʋn wa sʋɔr baar, ka a wʋ poturbo ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Sɩ Soro, wiil sɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ, nɩtãa lɛ a Jɔɔn na wiil a wʋ poturbo."
42011002	A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn ma wa sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn yɩ 'yɛr, Sɩ Sãa, sɩ kʋ naa a fʋ yuor tɩɩr. A fʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ wʋ wa.
42011003	Na fʋ kʋ sɩ a sɩ bɩbir jaa bʋ̃diir.
42011004	Vɛ̃ a sɩ maal dɛbɛ bar, bojũu sɩ mɩ vɛ̃n kʋ a bala jaa na maal sɩ a dɛɛr. Ta sɔɔ ka bɛɛr kaa nyɔɔ sɩ ɛ."
42011005	Be lɛ wʋ pãa 'yɛr kʋ ba. "Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ tara na baraa na wʋ wa ir chen a wʋ sɛ̃ tɩ̃sɔɔ bɩ̃ɩn tɩ 'yɛr, 'Pɛ̃ɛ ma jɔ̃ nɩ ŋmele,
42011006	bojũu n baraa ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ wa suu a tɩ̃sɔɔ nyãna tɩ n ba tara bon na maal kʋ wʋ ɛ.'
42011007	Ka wʋ gã be a die pɔ tɩ 'yɛr, 'Ta dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma ɛ, a pãn pɔɔ naa ka maa naa bibiir be gã, n kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ ir kʋ fʋ bon go ɛ.'
42011008	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, a wʋ baraa na ba sɔɔ ir kʋ wʋ a jɔ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋn chɛnɛ ara kpãkpãana, wʋn wa ir kʋ wʋ jɩ̃ a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ.
42011009	"Lɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ sʋɔr, Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ yɩ naa. Yɩ kaa yɩn nyɛ naa, yɩ kpoor a pãn wʋn yuo naa.
42011010	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sʋɔr, wʋn nyɛ naa, ka a 'lɔ mɩ na kaara nyɛ, ka a pãn mɩ yuo kʋ a 'lɔ na kpoor.
42011011	A yɩn na ɩ a sãamɩne, buor sʋɔ bie lɛ na sʋɔr wʋ jɩ̃m ka wʋ de waa kʋ wʋ.
42011012	Bɩɩ sʋɔr najɛl ka wʋ de lɔ̃ɔ kʋ wʋ?
42011013	Ala ɩ a yɩn gba na ɩ nɩdɛbɛ bɔ̃ɔn vɩla ma ɩ kʋ a yɩ bibiir, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an ɩ ka yɩ Sãa na be a saaju kʋ̃ de a Sɩɛ kʋ a bala na sʋɔr wʋ ɛ?"
42011014	Yesu dire naa a sɩdɛɛr na be daba yɔ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka wʋ ɩ wõo. A sɩdɛɛr na wa yi a daba 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka wʋ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ, ka nɛ'maa a nɩbɛ.
42011015	Tɩchɛ ka a bamɩne 'yɛrɛ, "A sɩdɛbɛ nãa Beeljebul lɛ wʋ de dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ."
42011016	Ka a bamɩne mɩ bɛɛr wʋ kaara na ba bʋɔrɔ jɩ̃nɛ na yi saaju.
42011017	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ban tɩɛrɛ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nãa jaa na jɛɛrɛ nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a wʋ nãa na sɔ̃ɔ naa. Yir nɩbɛ mɩ na ir jɛɛrɛ taa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'mataa kpɛ ɛ.
42011018	Lɛ mɩ lɛ, ala ɩ a Satan lɩɛb jɛɛrɛ nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ na ɩ ara? N 'yɛr naa nɩtɔ̃ bojũu yɩ 'yɛr ɩka a Beeljebul lɛ n de dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ.
42011019	Ala ɩ a Beeljebul lɛ n tara dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ, tɩ a bala na ɩ a yɩ poturbo bo lɛ ba tara dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ? A lɛ jũu, bala lɛ na ɩ a yɩ 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ.
42011020	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ lɛ n dire nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yire wiil yɩn ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ wa naa a yɩ sɛ̃.
42011021	"Gãdaa na gu a wʋ yir nɩ jɛɛr bomo, a wʋ bonsɩ maa dam ɛ.
42011022	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ wa wa naa na wʋ kpɛ̃mɛ gar wʋ, wʋn faan a wʋ jɛɛr bomo ala wʋn dɩɛl tɩ de a wʋ bonsɩ põn nɩbɛ.
42011023	"Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba be a n sɛ̃ ɛ, wʋ tara man nɩ 'yɛr, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba pʋɔ ma a sɩ kaala lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa ɛ, wʋ ma yɛ̃yɛl bar.
42011024	"Sɩdɛɛr ban wa dii bar ka wʋ yi nɩrɛ pɔ, wʋ ma chen dal pʋɔ ju tɩ bʋɔrɔ pɛ̃nfʋ jie, na waa nyɛ ɛ, na wʋ pãa wa 'yɛr, 'Ɩn lɩɛb kul a nɩrɛ 'lɔ pɔ ɩn yi tɩ chɛ bar.'
42011025	Wʋn wa lɩɛb wa, wʋ nyɛn a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kaara yir kaar ban pɩɩr tɩ chɔɔr wʋ sʋ̃.
42011026	Ka wʋ pãa tɩ bɔ sɩɩr ayopõi na tara putuo gar wʋ ka ba chen tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a be. Ka a daba pãa ɩ dɛɛr gar a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ be."
42011027	A nyãna lɛ a Yesu 'yɛrɛ ka a pɔɔ ŋme chɛlma be a nɩyɔɔ pɔ tɩ 'yɛr, "Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a fʋ ma 'lɔ na dɔɔ fʋ, nɩ a wʋ bɩr fʋn 'yɛn."
42011028	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, a bala na wõ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr na ba turo, bala lɛ ɩ a pʋpɛl dẽme."
42011029	A nɩbɛ na waara 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ka Yesu 'yɛr, "A dɩna nɩbɛ banyãna ɩn putudẽme tɩ bʋɔrɔ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ka a na ɩ jɩ̃nɛ, tɩchɛ ba kʋ̃ nyɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ɛ, ka a Jona jɩ̃nɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
42011030	Bojũu, lɛ a Jona na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ jɩ̃nɛ kʋ a Ninive dẽme, lɛ mɩ lɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na ɩ a jɩ̃nɛ kʋ a dɩna nɩbɛ.
42011031	A Siba Pɔɔ Nãa na yin a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar na wʋ wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ 'yɛr, bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ yi be a tẽtɛɛr wa chɛl a Nãa Solomon yɛ̃ 'yɛr, tɩchɛ yɩ kaa a 'lɔ na gar a Solomon ben ka.
42011032	A 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar Ninive nɩbɛ na ir 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ 'yɛr, bojũu ba lɩɛb ba tɩɛr a Jona na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ ba, yɩ kaa a 'lɔ na gar a Jona ben ka.
42011033	"Nɩrɛ jaa ba be na chʋm fɩ̃tɩn na wʋ sɔɔl bar ɛ, bɩɩ de laa kpa pɔɔ ɛ. Wʋ ma dɔɔl bar a dɔɔl fʋ jie, ka a bala na kpɩɛrɛ nyɛ a chãa.
42011034	A fʋ nɩbir ɩn a ɩ̃gãn fɩ̃tɩn. A fʋ nɩbie wa ɩ, a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa ma sɛɛn nɩ chãa. Tɩchɛ ala ba wa ɩ ɛ, a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa ma ɩn libe.
42011035	Yɩ kaara sʋ̃ ka a chãa 'lɔ na be a yɩ pɔ, taa lɩɛb libe ɛ,
42011036	A lɛ jũu, ala ɩ a chãa sɛɛn a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa ka a libe bɩ̃lãa jaa ba be be ɛ, wʋ jaa na ɩn chãa nɩtãa lɛ a fɩ̃tɩn na ma chaar fʋ a wʋ chãa."
42011037	Yesu na wa 'yɛr baar, Farasee nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ bʋɔl wʋ naa ka wʋ tɩ di bʋ̃diir, lɛ lɛ wʋ chen tɩ kpɛ jɩ̃nɛ a bʋ̃diir par.
42011038	Tɩchɛ ka a Farasee nɩrɛ jʋrɔ a Yesu ka a ɩ waa pɛɛ a ba pɛɛfʋ ɛ, ka nɛɛ 'maa wʋ.
42011039	Be lɛ a Soro pãa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Faa nyɛ, a yɩn Faraseemɩne ma pɛɛr naa a ŋmama nɩ a laar dũkur, tɩchɛ ka a yɩ pʋɔ sɛɛn fɔlfʋ nɩ putuo.
42011040	Jɔlɔ banyã, a ba ɩ a 'lɔ na maal a yõo 'lɔ lɛ mɩ maal a pʋɔ ɛ?
42011041	Tɩchɛ a ala na be a laa pʋɔm, yɩ de kʋ a nɔ̃n dẽme ka a bonsɩ a jaa pãa vɩɛlɛ kʋ yɩ.
42011042	"Nɛbier ben a yɩn Faraseemɩne sɛ̃, bojũu bʋ̃bile jaa yɩn da lɔ̃ɔn badʋʋ gba vaar, yɩ ma ir a da ŋmaa tɩ na yɩ ĩin vɩla maalfʋ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃fʋ bar. Ala lɛ yɩn taa irɛ na yɩ ta ĩin a ala na de nie bar ba maal ɛ.
42011043	Nɛbier ben a yɩn Faraseemɩne sɛ̃, bojũu yɩ nʋ̃ naa a nɩbɛrɛ jaa jie a yɩ lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie pɔ na yɩ mɩ nʋ̃ a daa pɔ puorfʋ.
42011044	Nɛbier ben a yɩ sɛ̃, bojũu yɩ kaara naa fɩka yar nɩbɛ na ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ do yʋɔrɔ."
42011045	Ka a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwile ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr, "Wiwile, a anyãna fʋn 'yɛr, sɩ jaa lɛ fʋ 'mataa tʋrɔ."
42011046	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "A yɩn Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɛbier ben a yɩ sɛ̃, bojũu yɩ ma tuon nɩbɛ tuor na tɩrɛ tɩ na yɩ maa ir a yɩ nubir gba tɩɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba ɛ.
42011047	Nɛbier ben a yɩ sɛ̃, bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ bala a yɩ sãamɩne na kʋ, yɩn lɛ mɛ a ba yar.
42011048	A lɛ yɩn maal din dãasɩɛ ɩka a yɩ sãamɩne lɛ. Bala lɛ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ka yɩ mɩ mɛ a ba yar.
42011049	A nɩtɔ̃ jũu lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ yɛ̃ sʋɔ 'yɛr, 'N tʋ̃n a n 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ nɩ a n nɩtʋ̃nsɩ a ba sɛ̃, ka ban ir bamɩne kʋ tɩ ge bamɩne.'
42011050	A lɛ jũu, yele tuon a yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ. A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ bala ban kʋ a kõr jaa, yɩn lɛ na yab a ba sãn.
42011051	Piel a Abel jɩ̃ɩ sɔ̃ɔ tɩ tãn a Jekariya ban kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie nɩ a puorfʋ jie chara pɔ. Ɔ̃ɔ, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a yɩn dɩna nɩbɛ lɛ na yab a jaa sãn.
42011052	Nɛbier ben a yɩn Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe sɛ̃, bojũu yɩn lɛ tara a bɔ̃ɔfʋ pãn bir, yɩn mɩ̃ɛ ba kpɩɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ pɔɔ var a bala na bʋɔrɔ a kpɛfʋ."
42011053	Yesu yin a be wʋn 'yɛr a anyãna, ka a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe kpãkpãana wʋ nɩ suur sʋrɔ nɩ wʋ 'yɛr yɔɔ.
42011054	Na ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ 'yɛr 'yɛr lɩɛb nyɔɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
42012001	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ lɛ, a nɩyɔɔ turo turo tire taa na ba nɛɛrɛ taa, ka Yesu piel kpãana a wʋ poturbo na wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a Faraseemɩne dãbɩl pɔ, ala lɛ ɩ a ba nɛɛr ayi.
42012002	Bon jaa ba be be na pɔɔ naa kʋ̃ wa yuo ɛ, bɩɩ sɔɔl ka ba kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔn ɛ.
42012003	Ala yɩn 'yɛr libe pɔ, na yin chãa pɔ, ka ba wõ naa, ka a ala yɩn bʋl 'yɛr be a die pɔ, ban mʋɔl 'yɛr be a gar ju.
42012004	"N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ a yɩn na ɩ a n barmɩne ɩka, yɩ ta joro a bala na kʋ a yɩ ɩ̃gãn ɛ, tɩ na ba kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ yele jaa ɩ ɛ.
42012005	Tɩchɛ ɩn wiil yɩ naa a 'lɔ yɩn na joro. Yɩ joro a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ɔ kʋ yɩ, tɩ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ lɔb yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a dɔɔyɛ jie. Ɔ̃ɔ, 'lɔ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ ɩka yɩ joro.
42012006	A ba ɩ kobsɩ ayi lɛ ba ma dãn tiitasɩ anũu ɛ? Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn maa ĩin a ba bʋ̃'yen bar ɛ.
42012007	Sɩrɛ jaa, Nãaŋmɩn sɔr a yɩ jukɔɔl a jaa bɔ̃ɔ, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, yɩ gar tiita yɔɔ.
42012008	"N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na wa 'yɛr chã a nɩbɛ niem, ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa a maa Nɩsaal Bie, 'lɔ lɛ n mɩ na 'yɛr chã ɩka, n bɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa a Nãaŋmɩn malakasɩ niem.
42012009	Tɩchɛ 'lɔ mɩ na chiir ma a nɩbɛ niem, 'lɔ lɛ n mɩ na chiir a Nãaŋmɩn malakasɩ niem.
42012010	Nɩrɛ jaa na 'yɛr 'yɛr kpɛ̃n a maa Nɩsaal Bie na chɛnɛ na nyɛ vɛ̃ kʋ fʋ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋ̃ nyɛ vɛ̃ kʋ fʋ ɛ.
42012011	Bala wa nyɔɔr yɩ chiin a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme sɛ̃, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a ɩ yɩ tɩɛr a lɛ yɩn na tɩ 'yɛr faa yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, bɩɩ a lɛ yɩn na 'yɛr ɛ.
42012012	Bojũu a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na wiil yɩ naa a lɛ yɩn na 'yɛr."
42012013	Ka nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ na be a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Wiwile 'yɛr a n yɛbɛ ka wʋ ɩ a sɩ põ a kpĩi bonsɩ."
42012014	A Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "Daba, an 'yɔ̃ɔ ma ɩka n ɩ 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ naa põnõ yɩ kpĩi bomo?"
42012015	Tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ kaara sʋ̃, na yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a bʋ̃yɔɔ bɔfʋ pɔ, nɩrɛ bʋ̃yɔɔ ba kʋrɔ wʋ nyɛvʋr ɛ."
42012016	Be lɛ wʋ lɔb a sʋkpa nyã kʋ ba, "Danãa kɔ̃ɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be, na wʋ kɔ chɛ yɔɔ jaa a wʋ puo pɔ.
42012017	Na wʋ piel tɩɛrɛ ɩka ŋmɩnɛ lɛ wʋn ɩ, 'Ɩn ba tara jie na bin a bonsɩ ɛ?'
42012018	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ ɩn ɩ, 'Ɩn ŋmɛr a bobo anyãna bar, tɩ naa mɛ bʋ̃bɛrɛ naa su a chi 'yɔ̃ɔn a bonsɩ a be.
42012019	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ n mɩ̃ɛ, ɩ̃gãn, pɛnɛ, n tara na bʋ̃yɔɔ ɩn bin kʋ n mɩ̃ɛ yuon kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔ sɔr ɛ. Ɩn dire naa, na n nyuro, na n chɩlɛ.'
42012020	Tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'Jɔl nyã, fʋn kpin a tɩ̃sɔɔ nyãna, tɩ a bonsɩ ala fʋn bin kʋ a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ, an lɛ na de?'
42012021	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ an be nɩrɛ jaa na bin bonsɩ kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, tɩ ba ɩ tara sʋɔ Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ."
42012022	Kaa Yesu pãa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "A lɛ jũu, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, yɩ ta waala a yɩ nyɛvʋr 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, 'yɛrɛ ɩka bo lɛ yɩn di ɛ. Bɩɩ waala ɩka bo lɛ yɩn su pɔɔ a ɩ̃gãn ɛ.
42012023	A nyɛvʋr gar naa a bʋ̃diir, ka a ɩ̃gãn mɩ gar a fɔɔr.
42012024	Yɩ kaa a gagasɩ, ba maa bʋr ɛ, bɩɩ ŋma ɛ, bɩɩ tara boor ma bin ɛ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ guolo ba. Yɩn, yɩ gar a lubil.
42012025	A yɩ buor sʋɔ lɛ na waal na wʋ wa de bɩbir bʋ̃'yen pʋɔ a wʋ nyɛvʋr pɔ?
42012026	Ala ɩ yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ a yelbile nyãna ɩ ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ tɩɛrɛ a ala na chɛ?
42012027	"Yɩ kaa nyɛ a lɛ a bonsɩ puul na ma nʋ̃ɔ. Ba maa tʋ̃ ɛ, bɩɩ wob fuu su ɛ, tɩchɛ a nãa Solomon gba nɩ a wʋ bʋ̃tarsɩ ba dɔ̃ɔ su fuu ka wʋ vɩɛlɛ gar naa ɛ.
42012028	Ala ɩ nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn ma pɩ̃ɛ a bonsɩ puul a mʋ̃ɔ pɔ ka a vɩɛlɛ a dɩna tɩchɛ ka a wɛr chaar ka a bũu di, wʋ kʋ̃ pɩ̃ɛ a yɩn gar a lɛ ɛ? Yɩn sɔɔfʋ na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ.
42012029	Yɩ ta ir nyãa 'yɔ̃ɔ a ala yɩn na di bɩɩ nyũ pɔ ɛ, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a yɩ pɩla ɔɔrɔ ɛ.
42012030	Nɩrɛ jaa, ala puor lɛ ba turo, tɩchɛ a yɩ Sãa bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka yɩ bʋɔrɔ naa a bonsɩ anyãna.
42012031	Yɩ de nie bɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ, ka anyãna a jaa wʋn den pʋɔ yɩ.
42012032	"Yɩn piir na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, bojũu a yɩ Sãa pʋɔ pɛl naa wʋn kʋ yɩ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ.
42012033	Yɩ da a yɩ bonsɩ de a libie põ nɔ̃n dẽme, yɩn tara naa a libie wʋʋr ala na ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ. Ka a yɩ bʋ̃tarsɩ be a saaju, naa kʋ̃ wur ɛ. Nãnyie kʋ̃ gbʋr be ɛ, kpolo ba be be na mʋʋ ɛ.
42012034	Bojũu, a jie a yɩ bʋ̃tarsɩ na be, be lɛ a yɩ nyãa mɩ ma gã.
42012035	"Yɩ chɔɔr yɩ mɩ̃ɛ gu tɩ chʋm a yɩ fɩ̃tɩnsɩ ka a lɩrɛ.
42012036	Yɩ kaara fɩka tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ na chɛlɛ a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ka wʋn yi a pɔɔ kulfʋ jie wa. 'Lɔ wa kpoor a pãn ban yuo wʋn a pãn ajienaa ka wʋ kpɛ.
42012037	An ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ banyãna a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wa nyɛ ba ka ba chɛnɛ jɛ̃ gu wʋ. Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka wʋn chɔɔr naa a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ka ba 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ a bʋ̃diir jie ka wʋ põ ba a bʋ̃diir.
42012038	An ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ bala a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wa nyɛ ban chɔɔr, ala ɩ gba ka tɩ̃sɔɔ põn lɛ bɩɩ, ka nɔrsɩ kõnõ naa.
42012039	Tɩchɛ yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a par, ɩka ala ɩ a yir sʋɔ bɔ̃ɔ naa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a nãnyie na waara, wʋ kʋ̃ sɔɔ ka a nãnyie kar a pãn tɩ kpɛ a yir ɛ.
42012040	A yɩn mɩ yɩ chɔɔr gu, bojũu a maa Nɩsaal Bie na lɩɛb wa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ yɩn ba lɛ tɩɛrɛ ma ɛ."
42012041	Ka a Pita sʋʋr wʋ, "N Soro, sɩn lɛ fʋ lɔb a sʋkpa nyã kʋ bɩɩ nɩrɛ jaa lɛ?"
42012042	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "An lɛ pãa ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a yɛ̃ sʋɔ, a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ kaara wʋ a yir, na wʋ kʋrɔ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ a ba bʋ̃diir a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ na sɛɛ?
42012043	An ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nyãna a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wa nyɛ wʋn ɩrɛ a lɛ.
42012044	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, wʋn vɛ̃n ka wʋ kaara a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa.
42012045	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nyãna tɩɛr a wʋ nyãa pɔ ɩka, a n nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kor a waa, tɩ piel pɔɔrɔ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ bala na be a yir, tɩ pãa ma di na wʋ nyũ buu.
42012046	A tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nyãna, a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wa dũu wʋ naa a bɩbir 'lɔ wʋn ba tɩɛrɛ nɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ. Wʋn ŋma wʋn jaa gbʋl gbʋl, tɩ lɔb wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na ba sɔɔ de pɔ ɛ.
42012047	A tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ 'lɔ na bɔ̃ɔ lɛ a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na bʋɔrɔ tɩ na waa chɔɔr tʋ̃n a lɛ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na bʋɔrɔ ɛ, wʋn nyɛn ŋmefʋ yɔɔ.
42012048	Tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ maal bɔr ban ŋme wʋn jaa bɩ̃lãa. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ ban kʋ yɔɔ ban bʋɔrɔ na yɔɔ yi a wʋ sɛ̃, fʋ̃ʋ nũu pɔ ban 'yɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ban sʋʋr yɔɔ.
42012049	"Bũu lɛ n waan ɩka n wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a wɛr pɔ, ɩn taa bʋɔrɔ naa ala ɩ a ben ta 'lɩrɛ.
42012050	Tɩchɛ n chɛnɛ tara yele ɩn na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ kaar ka a ɩ ma tɩɛr tɩ tãn ɩn na wa baar.
42012051	Yɩ maa tãan nɛbʋ̃'yen yele lɛ n waan a wɛr pɔ bɩɩ? Kai, n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ, tɩchɛ ootaa lɛ n waan.
42012052	An yi a dɩna nɩbɛ anũu na kpɩɛrɛ yir na ŋman jiir ayi. Ka ata jɛɛrɛ nɩ a ayi ka ayi mɩ jɛɛrɛ nɩ a ata.
42012053	Ban ooro nɩ taa, sãa na oon bie ka a bie mɩ oo a sãa, ka a ma oo a bipɔɔ ka a bipɔɔ mɩ oo a ma. Pɔɔ na oo naa a wʋ bidaba pɔɔ, ka a bidaba pɔɔ mɩ oo a wʋ sɩrɛ ma."
42012054	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a nɩyɔɔ bala, "Yɩn wa nyɛ julõjuur na ire a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ mʋrfʋ jie yɩ ma 'yɛr ɩka saa na wa naa, ka a ma ɩ a lɛ.
42012055	Yɩn wa nyɛ sɛsɛbɛ mɩ na furo duoro jũu, yɩ ma 'yɛr ɩka tʋl na wa naa. Ka a ma ɩ a lɛ.
42012056	A yɩn nɛɛr ayi dẽme banyãna. Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a tẽe nɩ a saaju 'yɛr ma 'yɛr, ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ a dɩna 'yɛr 'yɛr ɛ?
42012057	"Bo lɛ so ka yɩn mɩ̃ɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tɔɔr a lɛ na tor ɛ?
42012058	An ɩ a yɩn nɩ a yɩ sãn sʋɔ lɛ 'mataa chiine, yɩ mʋlɔ wʋ a sɔr pɔ, ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, wʋn de yɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ a 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ nũu pɔ, ka wʋ de yɩ kʋ a nɩpɔɔrɔ ka wʋ mɩ pɔɔ yɩ bar.
42012059	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, ala be ɩ a lɛ, faa be na wa yi ka faa yab a fʋ sãn baar ɛ."
42013001	Nɩbɛ bamɩne mɩ ben be a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, na ba pãa mana kʋrɔ a Yesu a lɛ a paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ Pilate na dɔ̃ɔ kʋ a Galilee dɔɔr bamɩne, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban be a bɔɔr lofʋ jie.
42013002	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ tɩɛr ɩka bala lɛ maal dɛɛr gar a Galilee nɩbɛ ba jaa, ala lɛ so ban di a dɔɔyɛ nyã bɩɩ?
42013003	A ba ɩ lɛ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩn ba wa lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr ɛ, yɩ mɩ na wɛ naa.
42013004	Bɩɩ a nɩbɛ pie nɩ aniin (18) bala a jiwõo 'lɔ na kar lo kʋ a Siloam, yɩ tɩɛr ɩka bala lɛ maal yeldɛɛr gar a bala jaa na kpɩɛrɛ a Jerusalɛm bɩɩ?
42013005	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩn mɩ baa lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr ɛ, yɩ mɩ na wɛ naa."
42013006	A sʋkpa nyã lɛ Yesu pãa lɔb kʋ ba, "Daba kɔ̃ɔ lɛ tara kɔ̃kɔ̃tɩɛ a wʋ puo pɔ, a wʋ wa chen ɩka wʋ tɩ kaa a tɩɛ wɔ̃n bɩɩ, tɩchɛ a tɩɛ ba wɔ̃ ɛ.
42013007	Be lɛ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ wʋn vɛ̃ ka wʋ kaara a puo, 'Bojũu, yuom ata nɩ nyã ɩn yɔ ka, ma bʋɔrɔ a wɔ̃mɔ̃ ɩka n pɔr tɩ ma wa bɔ faa. Ŋmaa wʋ lɔb, ŋmɩnɛ an ɩ ka wʋ pii a wɛr ara nɩ?'
42013008	Ka a 'lɔ na kaara a puo 'yɛr, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, bar wʋ ka n tuu jilʋ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ pʋɔr ka yuon waara,
42013009	'lɔ wa wɔ̃ go, tɩ 'lɔ ba wa wɔ̃ ɛ, ka n ŋmaa wʋ lɔb.' "
42013010	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar Yesu ben a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ wile ba,
42013011	be lɛ a pɔɔ be a sɩdɛbɛ na maal ka wʋ kab gʋ̃mɔ̃ yuom pie nɩ aniin (18), wʋ maa tʋ̃ɔ dɔl ɛ.
42013012	Yesu na nyɛ a pɔɔ a lɛ, wʋ bʋɔl wʋ naa ka wʋ wa a wʋ sɛ̃, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Pɔɔ, a fʋ baal bar fʋ naa."
42013013	Tɩ na wʋ pãa de a wʋ nũu dɔɔl a pɔɔ, ka a pɔɔ dɔl ajienaa na wʋ pɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn.
42013014	Tɩchɛ ka a suur kpɛ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir nɩdier Yesu na sãa a baalaa a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar jũu, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ, "Bibie ayʋɔb ben be ka nɩrɛ na de tʋ̃n tʋ̃mɔ̃, yɩ ma wa ka wʋ sãana yɩ a ber ala pɔ, yɩ ta ma waara a Pɛ̃nfʋ Daar ɛ."
42013015	Ka a Soro 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Yɩn nɛɛr ayi dẽme banyãna, a yɩ buor sʋɔ lɛ maa yuo a wʋ niin bɩɩ a wʋ bon chiin tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ kʋ̃ɔ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir ɛ?
42013016	Ka a pɔɔ nyãna na ɩ a Abraham bipɔɔ, a tɩɩ na lũ yuom pie nɩ aniin (18), a ba sɛɛ ɩka wʋ for a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar bɩɩ?"
42013017	Wʋn wa 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ ka a vĩ kpɛ a bala jaa na bɛrɛ wʋ a nɛɛ, tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ chɩlɛ a tʋ̃vɩɛlɛ ala wʋn tʋ̃.
42013018	A Yesu pãa 'yɛr, "Bo lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nyɛtãan? Bo lɛ ɩn de man?
42013019	Wʋ kaara fɩka kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ bir nɩrɛ na de bʋr a puo pɔ ka wʋ bul na wʋ ɩ tɩɛ, ka a lubil wa 'yɔ̃ɔ choor a wilsɩ ju."
42013020	Wʋ lɛ sʋʋr ban go, "Bo lɛ ɩn de a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ man?
42013021	Wʋ kaara fɩka dãbɩl pɔɔ na de 'yɔ̃ɔ jɔ̃ yɔɔ pɔ ka a ir vʋ̃."
42013022	Yesu wile naa nɩbɛ be a tẽbɛrɛ nɩ a tẽbil ala pɔ tɩ na wʋn chen Jerusalɛm.
42013023	Be lɛ a nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ sʋʋr wʋ, "N Soro, nɩbɛ bɩ̃lãa tɛɛ lɛ na nyɛ faafʋ bɩɩ?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba,
42013024	"Yɩ mɔ̃ tu a dɔ̃dɔ̃ bile pɔ kpɛ, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka nɩyɔɔ lɛ na mʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba kpɛ tɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ɛ.
42013025	A yir sʋɔ na wa ir pɔɔ a pãn var yɩ bar be a yõo, ka yɩ ara kpooro sʋɔrɔ, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, yuo sɩ a pãn.' Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ, 'N ba bɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɛ, bɩɩ a jie yɩn yi ɛ.'
42013026	Ka yɩ pãa 'yɛrɛ, 'Sɩn nɩ fʋ̃ʋ jaa 'mantaa di tɩ nyũ, a fʋ wiil sɩ be a sɩ tẽe sãlsɔɔ.'
42013027	Tɩchɛ ka wʋn 'yɛr, 'N ba bɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɛ, bɩɩ a jie yɩn yi ɛ, yɩ tɔɔ yi tɩ chɛ ma a yɩn na tʋ̃nɔ̃ a dɛbɛ.'
42013028	"Be lɛ yɩn kõnõ ɔɔrɔ a nyɩmɛ, yɩn wa nyɛ a Abraham, Isaakɩ nɩ Jekɔb nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ba jaa be a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a yɩn 'lɔ be a yõo.
42013029	Nɩbɛ na yin a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie, a mʋrfʋ jie, a jũu nɩ a par na ba wa jɩ̃nɛ dire be a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
42013030	Sɩrɛ jaa, nɩbɛ ben puor tɩ na ban wa de nie, ka a bala mɩ na be a niem mɩ wa be a puor."
42013031	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ lɛ a Faraseemɩne bamɩne wa a Yesu sɛ̃ wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Yi a ka chen jiyuo. A Hɛrɔd bʋɔrɔ na a fʋ kʋfʋ."
42013032	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen tɩ 'yɛr a mɔbaa 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, ɩn dii naa a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi ka n sãa a nɩbɛ baalsɩ a dɩna nɩ bio ka a dayere daar ka n baar a n tʋ̃mɔ̃.
42013033	Lɛ jaa an ɩ, ɩn chɛnɛ na chiine a dɩna nɩ bio nɩ a dayere. Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ kʋ̃ kpi ka Jerusalɛm ba lɛ ɛ.
42013034	"Gboo yɩn Jerusalɛm dẽme, yɩn lɛ ma kʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ tɩ lɔɔrɔ a bala Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ a yɩ sɛ̃ nɩ kʋsɩbɛ. N ma bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n kaal a fʋ bibiir 'mataa nɩtãa lɛ nʋ̃ɔ na ma kaal a wʋ bil 'mataa a wʋ pɩrɛ pɔ, tɩ yɩ maa sɔɔ ɛ.
42013035	Yɩ nyɛ, a yɩ yir na lɩɛb dakpolo, tɩ ka n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩ kõ lɛ nyɛ ma go ɛ, tɩ tãn a daar 'lɔ yɩn na 'yɛr, 'Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃!' "
42014001	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ daar, Yesu chen a Faraseemɩne nɩdiere ɩ̃sʋɔ yir difʋ jie ka ba jʋrɔ wʋ.
42014002	Be lɛ ka daba kɔ̃ɔ na tara a baal vʋ̃ naa ara a wʋ niem.
42014003	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ bɔ̃ɔnbɔ, "A tara na sɔr ka fʋn sãa nɩrɛ na bɩɛrɛ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir bɩɩ a ba tara sɔr ɛ?"
42014004	Tɩchɛ ka ba ɩ jaa gbulo, ka Yesu de a nũu dɔɔl a daba sãa a wʋ baal tɩ bar wʋ sɔr.
42014005	Tɩ na wʋ pãa sʋʋr ba, "Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ bie bɩɩ a wʋ nadar lon bulo pɔ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir, wʋ kʋ̃ chen tɩ ir wʋ fɔfɔɔ jaa bɩɩ?"
42014006	Baa lɛ tara 'yɛr na 'yɛr ɛ.
42014007	Yesu nyɛn a nɩbɛ bala ban bʋɔl ɩka ba wa di, ka ba tuur a nɩbɛrɛ jaa jiir jɩ̃nɛ, ka wʋ lɔb a sʋkpa nyã kʋ ba,
42014008	"Nɩrɛ wa bʋɔl fʋ pɔɔ kulfʋ jie, fʋ̃ʋ wa chen ta tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a nɩbɛrɛ jaa jie ɛ, amɩne wʋ bʋɔl nɩrɛ na gar fʋ ka wʋn wa.
42014009	Ala wa ɩ a lɛ, wʋn wa 'yɛr fʋ naa, 'Ir, ka a daba nyã jɩ̃nɛ a fʋ jaa jie.' Vĩ lɛ fʋn ir tɩ jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a puor.
42014010	Tɩchɛ bala wa bʋɔl fʋ, tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a puor, ka a 'lɔ na bʋɔl fʋ wa 'yɛr, 'N badaba wa jɩ̃nɛ ka a niem, be lɛ fʋn pãa vʋ̃ a fʋ taaba niem.'
42014011	Bojũu, nɩrɛ jaa na 'mɔɔrɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ saaju, Nãaŋmɩn na siir wʋ naa, 'lɔ mɩ na siir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn na 'mɔɔ wʋn saaju."
42014012	Ka Yesu pãa 'yɛr kʋ a 'lɔ na bʋɔl wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ wa bʋɔl nɩrɛ ɩka wʋ wa di, taa wa bʋɔlɔ a fʋ barmɩne, bɩɩ a fʋ yɛɛr, bɩɩ a fʋ bal nɩbɛ, bɩɩ a fʋ tɔ dẽme bala na ɩ tara dẽme ɛ. Ala ɩ fʋ ɩn a lɛ, ban bʋɔl fʋn daar kɔ̃ɔ tɩ yaa a sãn.
42014013	Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ wa bʋɔlɔ nɩbɛ ɩka ba wa di, bʋɔl a nɔ̃n dẽme, nɩ a gbɛrsɩ, nɩ a nɩbaalsɩ, nɩ a jɔ̃n.
42014014	Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na sʋ̃ʋ. Ban ba tara bon na yab fʋ ɛ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ na nyɛ sãyar a lɛ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ na wa ir a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋ ɛ."
42014015	Ka a bala na lɔ̃ɔ dire ɩ̃sʋɔ na wõ a nɩtɔ̃, na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "An ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n kʋ a 'lɔ na wa jɩ̃nɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ dire."
42014016	Be lɛ a Yesu lɔb a sʋkpa nyã, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ chɔɔrɔ na wʋ bʋɔlɔ nɩyɔɔ ɩka ba wa di.
42014017	A sɔ̃ɔ na wa ta, wʋ tʋ̃n a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɩka wʋ chen tɩ 'yɛr a bala wʋn bʋɔl ɩka wʋ maal yele a jaa baar.
42014018	Tɩchɛ ka a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa 'yɛr ɩka ba kʋ̃ nyɛ jie ɛ. Ka a 'lɔ ban dɔ̃ɔ ta ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'N dãn popaalaa naa chiine ɩka n tɩ kaa, n kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tɩ ɛ.'
42014019	Ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr, 'N dãn narkʋɔrsɩ pie naa jãna n kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tɩ ɛ.'
42014020	Ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr, 'Pɔɔ lɛ n de n kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tɩ be ɛ.'
42014021	"A tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ lɩɛb wa 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ kʋ a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, ka a suur kpɛ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃, 'Lɩɛb chen fɔfɔɔ jaa a tẽe sãlsɔɔ nɩ a kõkorsɩ pɔ, na fʋ tɩ bʋɔl a nɔ̃n dẽme, a gbɛrsɩ, jɔ̃n nɩ a nɩbaalsɩ waan.'
42014022	Ka a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ wa 'yɛr, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, n ɩ naa a lɛ fʋn 'yɛr ɩka n ɩ, tɩchɛ ka a jie chɛnɛ be be.'
42014023	Be lɛ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ pãa lɛ 'yɛr kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃, 'Yi chen a sɔɩ pɔ, nɩ a sɛɛr pɔ tɩ bʋɔl nɩbɛ waan ka n yir wa sɛɛ.
42014024	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ lɛ̃ maa ɛ.' "
42014025	Yesu nɩ a nɩyɔɔ 'mantaa chiine, ka wʋ lɩɛb kaa ba tɩ 'yɛr,
42014026	"Ala ɩ nɩrɛ na wa naa a n sɛ̃, na waa 'laar a wʋ sãa nɩ a wʋ ma, nɩ a wʋ pɔɔ, a wʋ bibiir, a wʋ yɛɛr nɩ a wʋ yɛpɔbɔ 'matãan a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nyɛvʋr ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a n poturo ɛ.
42014027	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na ba de a wʋ daa tuo turo nɩ ma ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a n poturo ɛ.
42014028	"Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ bʋɔrɔ na yir kpɛ̃ɛ mɛfʋ, a ba ɩ wʋn den nie jɩ̃nɛ guor kaa ala ɩ wʋ tara naa a libie na tʋ̃ɔ mɛn baar ɛ?
42014029	Na wʋ taa kpar a yir tɩ ba tʋ̃ɔ baar ɛ, ka a wʋ taaba nyɛ laara wʋ
42014030	'yɛrɛ, 'Jaal piel a mɛfʋ tɩ na waa baar ɛ.'
42014031	Bɩɩ nãbuor lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ tɩ jɛb a wʋ nãa tɔ sʋɔ na waa de nie jɩ̃nɛ kaa ɩka wʋn tʋ̃ɔ de a wʋ nɩbɛ turo pie (10,000) tɩ jɛb a 'lɔ na waara nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ turo lɩjɛr (20,000) ɔ?
42014032	Ala ɩ wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɛ, wʋn tʋ̃n nɩbɛ ka ba chen tɩ 'maal a nãa 'lɔ na chɛnɛ be a tɛɛr.
42014033	Lɛ mɩ lɛ, a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa baa bar a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a n poturo ɛ.
42014034	"Nyaar ɩ naa, tɩchɛ a wʋ nʋ̃ɔ wa baar, ŋmɩnɛ ban lɛ ɩ wʋ ka wʋ lɛ nʋ̃mɔ̃ go?
42014035	Wa vɩɛl kʋ a tãpuor tãna ɛ, ban lɔb bar. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor wõnõ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ wõ naa."
42015001	A lõpodierbe nɩ a tʋ̃dɛtʋ̃nbɔ lɔ̃ɔn taa na chɛl a Yesu 'yɛr.
42015002	Tɩchɛ ka a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe hũhũnõ 'yɛrɛ, "A daba nyã diere naa tʋ̃dɛtʋ̃nbɔ ka ba 'mataa dire."
42015003	A Yesu pãa lɔb a sʋkpa nyã kʋ ba,
42015004	"Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ tara na piir kɔbaa ka a bʋ̃'yen wa bɔr, a ba ɩ wʋn bar a kɔbaa forbir ala a pɛchiin baa pɔ, tɩ yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ a bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa wʋn wa tɩ nyɛ wʋ bɩɩ?
42015005	'Lɔ wa nyɛ a pɛr nʋ̃ɔ ma kpɛ wʋ naa ka wʋ 'mɔɔ dɔɔl bɔɔ ju
42015006	kulo nɩ a yir, tɩ pãa bʋɔlɔ a wʋ barmɩne nɩ a wʋ taaba lɔ̃ɔ taa tɩ 'yɛr, 'Yɩ pʋɔ ma chɩlɛ, bojũu n nyɛ naa a n pɛr 'lɔ na bɔr.'
42015007	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, chɩl kpɛ̃ɛ na ben a saaju a tʋ̃dɛtʋ̃nɔ̃ bʋ̃'yen na lɩɛb a wʋ tɩɛr gar a kɔbaa forbir bala na ba tara tɩɛr lɩɛb fʋ ɛ.
42015008	"Bɩɩ pɔɔ buor lɛ tara libibie pie ka ɩ̃sʋɔ bɔr, wʋ kʋ̃ chʋm bũu den saar pɩɩr a die wʋ jaa na wʋ wa tɩ nyɛ wʋ bɩɩ?
42015009	'Lɔ wa nyɛ wʋ, wʋ ma bʋɔl a wʋ barmɩne nɩ a wʋ taaba lɔ̃ɔ taa tɩ 'yɛr, 'Yɩ pʋɔ ma chɩlɛ, n nyɛ naa a n libir na bɔr.'
42015010	Lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, nʋ̃ɔ mɩ na kpɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn malakasɩ ala ɩ a tʋ̃dɛtʋ̃nɔ̃ bʋ̃'yen lɩɛb a wʋ tɩɛr."
42015011	Yesu chɛnɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ ba, "Daba lɛ tara wʋ dabil ayi.
42015012	Ka a bile sʋɔ wa 'yɛr kʋ a sãa, 'N sãa, põ a fʋ kpĩi bomo ir a n bon kʋ ma.' Ka a sãa de a wʋ kpĩi bomo põ ba.
42015013	A ba kor ɛ, ka a bile 'lɔ lɔ̃ɔ taa a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa yi chiin tẽyuo pɔ, na wʋ tɩ bũbur a bonsɩ sɔ̃ɔ a jaa bar.
42015014	Wʋn wa sɔ̃ɔ a jaa baar, ka a kɔ̃ lo a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ, ka a wõm piel kpɛ wʋ.
42015015	Wʋ chen a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ yir tɩ bɔ tʋ̃mɔ̃, ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ ma tʋ̃ wʋ ka wʋ chen a puo pɔ tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ dor bʋ̃diir.
42015016	A jɔ̃ pɛbɛ ala ma ɩrɛ wʋn vɔlaa ka wʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ 'wɔb tɩɩ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ jaa maa kʋ wʋ bon ɛ.
42015017	"Ka a yɛ̃ wa wʋ ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'N sãa tara na tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ a ŋmɩnɛ a ba ma di bʋ̃diir faa, tɩchɛ ka a maa wa kpire nɩ kɔ̃ ka?
42015018	Ɩn lɩɛb kul a n sãa sɛ̃ naa tɩ 'yɛr wʋ, n maal dɛɛr Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ nɩ a fʋ sɛ̃.
42015019	N ba lɛ chɛnɛ sɛɛ ka ban bʋɔl ma a fʋ bie ɛ, maal ma ka n ɩ a fʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɩ̃sʋɔ.'
42015020	Lɛ wʋ ir kulo a sãa sɛ̃. Tɩchɛ wʋn chɛnɛ be a nɩdaa waara, a sãa nyɛ wʋ naa ka nɩbaal kpɛ wʋ ka wʋ jotuor a bie kõr tɩ puor wʋ.
42015021	Ka a bidaba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'N sãa, n maal dɛɛr Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ nɩ a fʋ sɛ̃, n ba lɛ sɛɛn ka ban bʋɔl ma a fʋ bie go ɛ.'
42015022	Tɩchɛ ka a sãa 'yɛr kʋ a gbãgbaar, 'Yɩ pɔɔ fɔɔ tɩ de fuu nyã na vɩɛlɛ wa su wʋ, na yɩ de bɔ̃bile 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ a nubir pɔ, na yɩ de nafɔbɔ wa su wʋ.
42015023	Yɩ tɩ kaa nele na 'wɔr na yɩ waan wa kʋ ka sɩ 'wɔb tɩ chɩlɛ.
42015024	Bojũu a n bidaba nyãna dɔ̃ɔ kpi tɩ lɛ ir ɩ vʋr, wʋ dɔ̃ɔ bɔr tɩ sɩ lɛ nyɛ wʋ.' Ka ba piel chɩlɛ.
42015025	"Tɩchɛ ka a bidakpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ be a puo pɔ, na wʋ wa ir waara, wʋn wa gbʋrɔ a yir wʋ wõn bɩ̃nɛ nɩ chɛlsɩ.
42015026	Be lɛ wʋ bʋɔl a gbãgbaa ɩ̃sʋɔ na wʋ sʋʋr a yelnyɩnɛ na be be.
42015027	Ka a gbãgbaa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'A fʋ yɛbile lɛ wa ka a fʋ sãa ɩ a ba kʋ nel'wɔr jaa, bojũu wʋ nyɛn a wʋ bie na lɩɛb wa nɩ lãafɩɛ tɩ chɛnɛ kpɛ̃mɛ.'
42015028	A suur kpɛ a yɛkarma ka wʋ jɛ, waa kpɛ ɛ. Ka a sãa yi 'maala wʋ ɩka wʋ kpɛ.
42015029	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a sãa, 'Nyɛ lɛ ɩn wõnõ a fʋ toor naa tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ fʋ a yuom anyãna a jaa, n ba gɔ̃ɔ fʋ nɛɛ jaa ɛ. Tɩchɛ faa mɩ wa kʋ ma bule gba ɩka, n mɩ kʋ ka maa nɩ a n barmɩne mɩ 'mataa di tɩ chɩlɛ ɛ.
42015030	Tɩchɛ a fʋ bibawõno nyãna na de a fʋ bonsɩ yin ka a 'lɔ nɩ a pɔɔ baar tɩ 'mataa sɔ̃ɔ bar, tɩ lɩɛb wa a yir ka fʋ ir kʋ nel'wɔr kʋ wʋ.'
42015031	Ka a sãa 'yɛr, 'Fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ, fʋ ben a n sɛ̃, ka a bomo a jaa ɩn tara ɩ a fʋ bonsɩ.
42015032	Tɩchɛ a sɛɛ naa ka sɩn dɩ̃ɛnɛ na sɩ chɩlɛ bojũu a fʋ yɛbile nyãna dɔ̃ɔ kpi tɩ lɛ ɩ vʋr go, na wʋ dɔ̃ɔ bɔr tɩ sɩ lɛ nyɛ wʋ.' "
42016001	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo ɩka, "Taraa sʋ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be, na wʋ tara nɩrɛ na kaara wʋ a bonsɩ, na wʋ pʋ̃pʋrɔ bara.
42016002	Ka wʋ bʋɔl wʋ waan wa sʋʋr, 'N wõn ban 'yɛrɛ a fʋ 'yɛr yʋɔrɔ nɩ, man a lɛ fʋn tʋ̃ kʋ ma, bojũu fʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ.'
42016003	Ka a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, 'Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ɩn pãa ɩ a pʋ̃pãanyã? A n nɩkpɛ̃ɛ faa man a tʋ̃mɔ̃, n mɩ ba lɛ kpɛ̃mɛ na tʋ̃ɔ kɔ ɛ, a mɩ na ɩn vĩ ɩn na sʋɔrɔ.
42016004	N bɔ̃ɔ lɛ ɩn na ɩ maa ba lɛ wa tara tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka nɩbɛ chɛnɛ de ma a ba yie.'
42016005	Be lɛ wʋ bʋɔl a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sãma dẽme ba jaa na wʋ sʋʋr a 'lɔ na de nie, 'A ŋmɩnɛ lɛ fʋ di a n nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sãn?'
42016006	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'Kãlaar kɔbaa (100) lɛ n di a sãn.' Ka a 'lɔ na kaara a bonsɩ 'yɛr, 'De a gãn nyãna jɛn fɔɔ jaa na fʋ sɛb lɩjaayi nɩ pie (50).'
42016007	Tɩ na wʋ lɛ sʋʋr a ayi sʋɔ, 'A ŋmɩnɛ fʋ mɩ di a n nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sãn?' Ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'Chi bɔtɔr kɔbaa (100) sãn lɛ n di.' Ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'De a fʋ gãn na fʋ sɛb lɩjaa naar 'yɔ̃ɔ (80).'
42016008	Ka a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ dãn a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nyãna na ba tara yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, bojũu wʋ tɩɛr nɩdaar. A wɛr nyã nɩbɛ tara na yɛ̃ a ba taaba jie gar a chãa nɩbɛ.
42016009	"N 'yɛr na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, yɩ de a wɛr nyã bʋ̃tarsɩ na yɩ ŋman barmɩne ala wa baar, Nãaŋmɩn na de yɩn kpɛ̃n a yir kpo kpo 'lɔ pɔ.
42016010	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bʋ̃bile, wʋn tara naa yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bʋ̃yɔɔ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa mɩ na ba tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bʋ̃bile ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ mɩ tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bʋ̃yɔɔ ɛ.
42016011	Ala ɩ yaa tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a wɛr bʋ̃tarsɩ ɛ, an lɛ na sɔɔ de a yelmɩ̃ɛ bomo kʋ yɩ?
42016012	Ala ɩ yaa tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ bon ɛ, an lɛ na kʋ yɩ a yɩ bon?
42016013	Gbãgbaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ kʋ nɩbɛrɛ ayi ɛ, wʋn nʋ̃n ɩ̃sʋɔ tɩ 'laar ɩ̃sʋɔ, bɩɩ wʋn wõnõ na ɩ̃sʋɔ toor tɩ ba wõnõ ɩ̃sʋɔ toor ɛ. Yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ libie ɛ."
42016014	A Faraseemɩne na nʋ̃ libie na wõ a lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr, ka ba laara wʋ.
42016015	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ma maal yɩ mɩ̃ɛ nɩtorsɩ a nɩbɛ niem, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn bɔ̃ɔn a yɩ tɩɛr. Bon 'lɔ nɩbɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃chiiraa.
42016016	"A Mosesɩ Nɛɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ 'yɛr wa tãn a Jɔɔn sɔ̃ɔ. An yi a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋ jaa, ba 'yɛr naa a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr sʋ̃n ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mʋɔrɔ wʋ sɔr, ɩka wʋ kpɛ.
42016017	An ɩn kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ kʋ a saaju nɩ a tẽe ka a po tal, gar a Nɛɛ 'yɛr bir na yi lo.
42016018	Nɩrɛ jaa na dii a wʋ pɔɔ bar tɩ kul pɔɔ yuo, wʋ maal dɛɛr, ka a daba 'lɔ mɩ na kul a pɔɔ a sɩrɛ na dii bar, mɩ maal dɛɛr.
42016019	"Tara sʋɔ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be, na wʋ ma su kparsɩ nɩ fuu pɩɛl na wʋ dire bʋ̃nʋ̃n bɩbir jaa.
42016020	Ka a sʋsʋɔrɔ kɔ̃ɔ yuor na di Lajarusɩ mɩ be be na ɩ natɩnara ma jɩ̃nɛ a tara sʋɔ dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ.
42016021	Na wʋ ma bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ nyɛ a bʋ̃di pʋr pʋr ala a tara sʋɔ na dire ka a ŋmara loro, ka a baar gba ma wa lɛnɛ a wʋ natɩɛ.
42016022	A sʋsʋɔrɔ nyãna wa kpi naa, ka a malakasɩ wa de wʋ chiine tɩ bin a Abraham sɛ̃. Ka a tara sʋɔ 'lɔ mɩ wa kpi ka ba ũu wʋ.
42016023	"A be a kpĩisɩ tẽe, ka a ɩ dɔɔyɛ jie lɛ, ka wʋ gbã nyɛ Abraham tɛɛr jaa ka a Lajarusɩ jɩ̃nɛ a wʋ lõboor.
42016024	Be lɛ wʋ bʋɔl, 'N sãa Abraham, kaa n nɩbaal tɩ na fʋ tʋ̃ a Lajarusɩ ka wʋ 'me kʋ̃ɔ nɩ nubir wa 'maan ma jãlbir, bojũu a wõnõ ma naa ka a bũu pɔ.'
42016025	Tɩchɛ ka a Abraham 'yɛr, 'N bie, tɩɛr kaa fʋn dɔ̃ɔ be a wɛr pɔ dire nʋ̃ɔ, tɩchɛ ka a Lajarusɩ mɩ dire dɔɔyɛ, pʋ̃pãanyã, wʋ mɩ dire naa a nʋ̃ɔ tɩchɛ ka fʋ mɩ dire a dɔɔyɛ.
42016026	A nyã gba ba ɩ yele ɛ, a bɔɔ kpɛ̃ɛ nyã na be a sɩ chara pɔ, ka a bala na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba yi a ka tɩ a yɩ sɛ̃ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɛ, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ yi a be tɩ mɩ wa a sɩ sɛ̃ ɛ.'
42016027	"Ka wʋ lɔb nũu 'yɛr, 'Yãayãaabɩlɛ lɛ n sʋɔrɔ, n sãa, tʋ̃ a Lajarusɩ ka wʋ kul a be a sãa yir,
42016028	n tara na yɛɛr anũu wʋ tɩ kpãa ba ka ba taa ɩrɛ mɩ wa wa a dɔɔyɛ nyã pɔ ɛ.'
42016029	Ka Abraham 'yɛr, 'Mosesɩ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ a lɛ ban sɛb bin ben a ba sɛ̃, ba chɛlɛ a ala ban 'yɛrɛ.'
42016030	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'Kai n sãa Abraham, ala ɩ nɩrɛ lɛ ir a kũu pɔ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba ban lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr.'
42016031	Ka a Abraham 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'Ala ɩ ba kʋ̃ chɛl a lɛ a Mosesɩ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na 'yɛr lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr ɛ, nɩrɛ sɔɔ ir kũu pɔ tɩ 'yɛr an ɩn pɔrɔ.' "
42017001	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "Yelsɩ ala na vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ ɩ bier ben be na wa, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jie an tu wa ben pɔ'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ pɔ.
42017002	A nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, bala 'mɔɔ nɩɛr lũ yɔɔl a nyĩe pɔ daa lɔb a man kʋ̃ɔ pɔ, ala sa wʋn na vɛ̃ ka a bʋ̃bil banyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩ bier.
42017003	Yɩ guro yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, ala ɩ fʋ yɛbɛ maal fʋn dɛɛr gɔ̃ wʋ, 'lɔ wa de a bɔrfʋ vɛ̃ kʋ wʋ.
42017004	Ala ɩ a bɩbir bʋ̃'yen pɔ lɛ wʋ maal fʋ dɛɛr gbɛɛ ayopõi tɩ mɩ lɩɛb wa a gbɛɛ ayopõi wa de bɔrfʋ, vɛ̃ kʋ wʋ."
42017005	Ka a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩ Soro, pʋɔ sɩ sɔɔfʋ."
42017006	Ka a Soro 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn tara sɔɔfʋ jaa pʋʋr fɩka kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ bir, yɩn tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a tɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyãna, 'Vʋ̃ɔ tɩ ba man pɔ, ka wʋ tu a lɛ yɩn 'yɛr.'
42017007	"Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ tara na gbãgbaa ka wʋ kʋɔrɔ bɩɩ ŋmaara piir, 'lɔ wa yi a tʋ̃mɔ̃ jie wa, fʋn 'yɛr wʋ naa ɩka wʋ wa jɩ̃nɛ di ɔ?
42017008	A ba ɩ fʋn 'yɛr wʋ naa, 'Maal a bʋ̃diir fɔɔ na fʋ chɔɔr a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ wa ara gu ma, ka n di tɩ nyũ baar ka fʋ mɩ pãa di tɩ nyũ ɛ.'
42017009	Wʋn puor naa a gbãgbaa nyãna wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ maal bɩɩ?
42017010	A yɩn mɩ lɛ lɛ, yɩn wa maal ala a jaa Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ, yɩn 'yɛr naa, 'Saa sɛɛn ɛ, gbãgbaar lɛ sɩ ɩ na sɩ maal a lɛ na ɩ a sɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃.' "
42017011	Yesu den a sɔr chiine a Jerusalɛm, wʋ kpɛ̃n a Samariya nɩ a Galilee chara pɔ.
42017012	Na wʋ chiine kpɛ a tẽbile ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, ka a kɔ̃kɔ̃n pie tuor wʋ a be. Ba ara na tɛɛr jaa
42017013	tɩ gboolo bʋɔlɔ, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ Yesu, kaa sɩ nɩbaal."
42017014	Wʋn nyɛ ba a lɛ, na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen tɩ wiil a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlorbo." Ban chen a lɛ, ka a ɩ ba sa naa.
42017015	A ba ɩ̃sʋɔ na nyɛ ka a ɩ wʋ sa naa, wʋ lɩɛb wa de nɛkpɛ̃ɛ na wʋ pɛɛrɛ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn.
42017016	Wʋ lon kpa a Yesu gbɛɛ par tɩ puor wʋ, Samariya lɛ wʋ yi.
42017017	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr, "A ba ɩ pie lɛ sa ɛ? Ka nyɩnɛ a pie forbir be?
42017018	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba lɩɛb wa ɩka wʋ wa puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan ka a sãan nyã ba lɛ ɛ."
42017019	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ir kulo, a fʋ sɔɔfʋ sa fʋ naa."
42017020	A Faraseemɩne lɛ sʋʋr naa Yesu ɩka dabor lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ na wa, ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ kʋ̃ wa ka ba bɔ̃ɔn ɛ.
42017021	Bɩɩ ka nɩbɛ 'yɛr, yɩ nyɛ wʋ ka, bɩɩ yɩ nyɛ wʋ kasɛn, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ ben a yɩ pɔ."
42017022	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo, "Sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ waara na a yɩn wa bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ nyɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie nɩ nɩbir, tɩchɛ yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ ma ɛ.
42017023	Nɩbɛ na 'yɛr yɩ naa, 'Kasɛn lɛ wʋ be,' bɩɩ 'Ka lɛ wʋ be.' Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa joro turo ba chiine be ɛ.
42017024	A maa Nɩsaal Bie bɩbir na kaara naa fɩka a saa na ma nyɩɩr a saaju yi a lõboor nyã tɩ gbem a lõboor ɩ̃sʋɔ.
42017025	Tɩchɛ ɩn den nie di dɔɔyɛ yele yɔɔ jaa pɔ, ka a dɩna nɩbɛ tɔr ma.
42017026	"Lɛ an dɔ̃ɔ kaara a Nowa sɔ̃ɔ, lɛ mɩ lɛ an kaara a maa Nɩsaal Bie sɔ̃ɔ.
42017027	Nɩbɛ dire naa na ba nyuro ka dɔɔr nɩ pɔbɔ kulo taa, tɩ tãn a bɩbir 'lɔ a Nowa na kpɛ a gbor kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ, ka a kʋ̃ɔ paal wa sɔ̃ɔ ba jaa bar.
42017028	"Lɛ mɩ lɛ a kaara a Lotɩ sɔ̃ɔ, nɩbɛ dire naa, na ba nyuro, na ba daara lɩɛb daara, na ba bʋrɔ na ba mɩɛrɛ nɩ yie.
42017029	Tɩchɛ a bɩbir 'lɔ a Lotɩ nɩ wa yi a Sodom bũu nɩ kʋsɩlirsɩ yin saaju lo pɔɔ a nɩbɛ ka ba jaa kpi.
42017030	Lɛ lɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie bɩbir mɩ na kaara.
42017031	"A bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, nɩrɛ na be a wʋ gar ju, ka a wʋ bonsɩ be a die pɔ, wʋ kʋ̃ suu tɩ de ɛ. Lɛ mɩ lɛ nɩrɛ na be puo pɔ kʋ̃ kul tɩ de bon ɛ.
42017032	Yɩ tɩɛr a Lotɩ pɔɔ.
42017033	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ faa a wa nyɛvʋr na bɔr wʋ naa, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na lɔb a wʋ nyɛvʋr bar, wʋn tara wʋ naa.
42017034	"N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a tɩ̃sɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, nɩbɛ ayi na gãn gaa jie, ka a Nãaŋmɩn wa de bʋ̃'yen tɩ chɛ bʋ̃'yen bar.
42017035	Ka a pɔbɔ ayi nɩɛnɛ jɔ̃, ka a Nãaŋmɩn de bʋ̃'yen tɩ chɛ bʋ̃'yen bar.
42017036	Dɔɔr ayi mɩ na ben puo pɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn wa de ɩ̃sʋɔ tɩ chɛ bʋ̃'yen bar."
42017037	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Sɩ Soro, nyɩnɛ?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Jie bʋ̃kũu na be, be lɛ sɩdumosɩ ma loro."
42018001	Yesu pãa lɔb sʋkpa kʋ a wʋ poturbo na wʋ wiil ba a lɛ ban na sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn taa baala ɛ.
42018002	Wʋ 'yɛr naa, "A tẽe kɔ̃ɔ pɔ, 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ kɔ̃ɔ dɔ̃ɔ be be, waa joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, waa mɩ kaara nɩrɛ nɩbaal ɛ.
42018003	Ka a pɔɔ kʋɔr kɔ̃ɔ mɩ be be a tẽe pɔ, na wʋ ma waara a wʋ sɛ̃ wa 'yɛrɛ, ''Yɛr faa ma a n sãn sʋɔ sɛ̃.'
42018004	Bojũu, gbɛɛ aŋmɩnɛ jaa lɛ wʋ ma tɔr, tɩ wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, 'N gba ba joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, bɩɩ kaara nɩrɛ nɩbaal lɛ.
42018005	Tɩchɛ bojũu, a pɔɔ kʋɔr nyãna na yʋɔrɔ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma, ɩn tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ka wʋ ta yʋɔrɔ bala ma ɛ.' "
42018006	Ka a Soro 'yɛr, "Yɩ nyɛ lɛ a 'yɛr tɔɔr filefile nyã na 'yɛr.
42018007	Nãaŋmɩn mɩ kʋ̃ 'yɛr faa a wʋ nɩ-irsɩ na kõnõ kʋrɔ wʋ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ jaa ɛ? Bɩɩ wʋn lɩɛrɛ ban bara?
42018008	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na tɔɔr a ba 'yɛr fɔɔ jaa kʋ ba. A maa Nɩsaal Bie wa lɩɛb wa a wɛr pɔ, ɩn nyɛn nɩbɛ ka ba tara sɔɔfʋ ɔ?"
42018009	Yesu lɛ lɔb sʋkpa de man a nɩbɛ bamɩne na tɩɛr ɩka ba ɩn nɩtorsɩ tɩ kaara a ba taaba pɔrɔ.
42018010	"Nɩbɛ ayi lɛ dɔ̃ɔ do a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ɩka ba tɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn. Ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩn Farasee nɩrɛ, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ ɩ lõpodiere.
42018011	Ka a Farasee nɩrɛ 'lɔ ir ara, tɩ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ nɩ, 'Nãaŋmɩn n puor fʋn yãan, nɩ ɩn ba kaara a nɩbɛ bamɩne kaar ɛ, nɩfarba, tʋ̃dɛtʋ̃nbɔ, sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ, bɩɩ a lõpodiere nyã kaar gba ɛ.
42018012	Maa 'lɔ, n ma gal kɔ̃ gbɛɛ ayi daa jaa pɔ, n bonsɩ pie jaa pɔ, n ma ir naa a bʋ̃'yen.'
42018013	Tɩchɛ ka a lõpodiere 'lɔ mɩ ara tɛɛr jaa na wʋ 'wor nuur, waa 'la dʋɔ kaa saaju ɛ, tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, 'Nãaŋmɩn kaa n nɩbaal, yelbe-ɩrɛ lɛ n ɩ.'
42018014	A lõpodiere nyã yele tor naa a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, ka wʋ lɩɛb kul gar, a Farasee nɩrɛ 'lɔ. Bojũu nɩrɛ jaa na 'mɔɔrɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ saaju, Nãaŋmɩn na siir wʋ naa, tɩ nɩrɛ nyã mɩ na siir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn na 'mɔɔ wʋn saaju."
42018015	Nɩbɛ dɔ̃ɔ waara nɩ bibibil a Yesu sɛ̃ ɩka wʋ sɩɩr ba, ka a poturbo na nyɛ a lɛ na ba mĩi 'yɔ̃ɔ ba.
42018016	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu bʋɔl a bibiir ka ba wa a wʋ sɛ̃, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ bar a bibiir sɔr ka ba wa a n sɛ̃, na yɩ ta ŋmaa ba sɔr ɛ, bojũu banyãna taaba lɛ so a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ.
42018017	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba wa de a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nɩtãa a bibibile nyãna kaar ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ be ɛ."
42018018	A nɩdiere kɔ̃ɔ sʋʋr a Yesu, "Wiwiilsʋ̃, bo lɛ ɩn ɩ naa nyɛ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ?"
42018019	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ fʋ bʋɔl ma nɩsʋ̃? Nɩrɛ jaa ba ɩ nɩsʋ̃ ka Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
42018020	Fʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa a Nãaŋmɩn Nɛɛ. Taa sɛ̃nɛ ɛ, taa kʋrɔ nɩrɛ ɛ, taa juro ɛ, taa ŋmaa jir kara 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ ɛ, na fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ sãa nɩ a fʋ ma."
42018021	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "A anyãna a jaa lɛ n turo a n bile sɔ̃ɔ wa tãn dɩna."
42018022	Yesu na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A chɛ fʋn yelbʋ̃'yen, tɩ da a fʋ bonsɩ a jaa, de põ nɔ̃n dẽme ka a fʋ tara bomo be a saaju, tɩ na fʋ pãa wa turo ma."
42018023	A daba na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa, bojũu tara sʋɔ lɛ wʋ ɩ.
42018024	Yesu kaa wʋn tɩ 'yɛr, "An ɩn kpɛ̃ɔ a tara sʋɔ na kpɛ Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
42018025	Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, an ɩn kɔ̃mɔ̃kɔ̃mɔ̃ nyɔɔma na kpɛ kparpĩi bɔɔ pɔ, gar tara sʋɔ na kpɛ Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
42018026	Ka a bala na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ sʋʋr a Yesu, "An lɛ na pãa nyɛ faafʋ?"
42018027	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Ala na ɩ tuo nɩrɛ sɛ̃, Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ yele jaa ba ɩ tuo ɛ."
42018028	A Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Sɩn bar bonsɩ a jaa, tɩ wa turo fʋ."
42018029	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ na bar a wʋ yir, bɩɩ pɔɔ, bɩɩ yɛɛr, bɩɩ a wʋ sãa naa ma, bɩɩ bibiir a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ jũu,
42018030	wʋn nyɛn dɔɔl taa a dɩna nɩ daar kɔ̃ɔ na wa lɔɔn nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ."
42018031	Yesu tɔɔn a Pie nɩ Ayi yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ, tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Sɩ ben duoro a Jerusalɛm, ala a jaa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na sɛb 'yɛr a maa Nɩsaal Bie 'yɛr, an tɩ ɩ naa.
42018032	Ban tɩ nyɔɔ man kʋ a nɩbɛ bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka ba la ma, tʋrɔ ma, na ba chɩr nataar 'yɔ̃ɔ ma, na ba ge ma, tɩ kʋ ma.
42018033	Ka a ber ata daar ka n ir ɩ vʋr go."
42018034	A poturbo ba bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna wʋn 'yɛr par bɩ̃lãa jaa ɛ. A liin ba jaa, baa bɔ̃ɔ a ala wʋn 'yɛrɛ ɛ.
42018035	Yesu na wa gbʋrɔ a Jeriko, jɔ̃ɔ jɛ̃n be a sɔr kõkoor na wʋ sʋɔrɔ.
42018036	Wʋn wa wõ a nɩyɔɔ na chiine tala, a wʋ sʋrɔ, ɩka bo lɛ ɩrɛ.
42018037	Ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Yesu na yi Najaretɩ lɛ tala."
42018038	A wʋ gboolo, "Yesu, David Bidaba, kaa a n nɩbaal."
42018039	Ka a bala na de a nie tãn wʋ 'yɛrɛ pɔɔ a nɛɛ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ chɛnɛ gboolo bʋɔlɔ, "Yesu, David Bidaba, kaa n nɩbaal."
42018040	Ka Yesu tɛɛ ara tɩ 'yɛr ɩka ba tara a daba waan. Lɛ a jɔ̃ɔ na wa gbʋr a Yesu ka wʋ sʋʋr wʋ,
42018041	"Bo lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka n ɩ kʋ fʋ?" Ka a jɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, "N Soro n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n nyɛrɛ."
42018042	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Nyɛrɛ a fʋ sɔɔfʋ sa fʋ naa."
42018043	Ajienaa ka a ɩ wʋ nyɛrɛ naa, na wʋ dãna Nãaŋmɩn turo nɩ a Yesu. A nɩbɛ ba jaa na wa nyɛ a lɛ, ba mɩ dãna naa a Nãaŋmɩn.
42019001	Yesu kpɛ̃n a Jeriko tẽe pɔ tala.
42019002	Ka a daba kɔ̃ɔ be be ban bʋɔlɔ Jakiyas, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a lõpodierbe nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wʋ ɩ tara sʋɔ.
42019003	Wʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ nyɛ Yesu nɩ nɩbir, tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ waa, a wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ wʋ ɛ, bojũu nɩŋmaa lɛ wʋ ɩ.
42019004	Be lɛ wʋ de nie jo chen tɩ do kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ tɩɛ ju ɩka wʋ nyɛ a Yesu an ɩ a be lɛ wʋ tu tala.
42019005	Yesu na wa ta a tɩɛ pĩlem, wʋ dʋɔn bʋɔl wʋ, "Jakiyas wa suu fɔɔ, a fʋ yir lɛ ɩn gã dɩna."
42019006	Ka a Jakiyas suu fɔɔ jaa na wʋ tuor de a Yesu nɩ pʋpɛl.
42019007	A nɩbɛ ba jaa nyɛn a lɛ na ba piel hũhũnõ 'yɛrɛ, "Wʋ ben na tɩ kpɛ a yelbe-ɩrɛ nyãna sãan."
42019008	Tɩchɛ ka a Jakiyas ir ara tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Nyɛ n Soro, ɩn põ naa a n bʋ̃tarsɩ ŋmaa, naa kʋ a nɔ̃n dẽme, ala ɩ n mɩ fɔl nɩrɛ jaa bon, ɩn yab a lɛ dɔɔl gbɛɛ anaar."
42019009	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Dɩna faafʋ wan a yir nyã pɔ, bojũu a daba nyã mɩ ɩn a Abraham bie.
42019010	Bojũu a maa Nɩsaal Bie wa naa ɩka n wa bɔ na n faa a bala na bɔr."
42019011	Ban chɛlɛ a anyãna ka wʋ lɔb sʋkpa kʋ ba, bojũu ba gbʋrɔ naa a Jerusalɛm ka nɩbɛ tɩɛr ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ na tɔɔn daa yi ajienaa.
42019012	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nãbie ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ ir na chen a tẽtɛɛr ɩ̃sʋɔ ka ba tɩ su wʋ nãa, ka wʋ lɩɛb wa.
42019013	Na wʋ bʋɔl a wʋ gbãgbaar pie na wʋ de a sɛlbie pie na wʋ kʋ ba tɩ 'yɛr, 'Yɩ de a libie anyãna tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ, wa tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn na lɩɛb wa.'
42019014	Tɩchɛ ka a wʋ tẽe dẽme 'laar wʋ, ir nɩbɛ tʋ̃ wʋn chen baar ka ba tɩ 'yɛr ɩka, 'Baa bʋɔrɔ a daba nyã ɩka wʋ wa ɩ a ba nãa ɛ.'
42019015	"Wʋ din a nãa na wʋ lɩɛb wa a wʋ tẽe, wʋ wa tʋ̃n bʋɔl a wʋ gbãgbaar bala wʋn kʋ a libie ka ba wa a wʋ sʋʋr kaa a lɛ ban tʋ̃n a libie.
42019016	A 'lɔ na de nie wa 'yɛr naa, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, a fʋ libir dɔɔn pie dɔɔl.'
42019017	Ka a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr, 'Fʋ maal vɩla fʋn ben tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bʋ̃bile nyã, ɩn vɛ̃ naa ka fʋ kaara tẽn pie.'
42019018	A ayi sʋɔ wa 'yɛr, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, a fʋ libir mɩ dɔɔn anũu dɔɔl.'
42019019	Ka a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr, 'Mɩ kaara tẽn anũu.'
42019020	"Ka ata sʋɔ mɩ wa 'yɛr, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyɛ a fʋ libir ɩn lũ 'yɔ̃ɔ fɔbaa pɔ bin.
42019021	N joro fʋn dãbɩ̃ɛ, bojũu a fʋ yele kpɛ̃mɛ naa. Fʋ ma den a jie 'lɔ fʋn ba bin ɛ, na fʋ ŋma a jie 'lɔ fʋn ba bʋr ɛ.'
42019022	Ka a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr, 'A fʋ nɛɛ 'yɛrbie lɛ ɩn de tɔɔr a fʋ 'yɛr, gbãgbadɛɛr lɛ fʋ ɩ. Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a n yele kpɛ̃mɛ naa, ma de a be ɩn ba bin ɛ, na n ma ŋmara a jie 'lɔ ɩn ba bʋr ɛ.
42019023	Bo lɛ so ka faa de a n libir tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a be a libie binfʋ jie ɛ, ɩn ben ta wa, n kʋ̃ naa de ka bon dɔɔl ɛ?'
42019024	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a bala na ara a be, 'Yɩ faa a libir 'lɔ a wʋ sɛ̃, na yɩ kʋ a 'lɔ na tara a libie pie.'
42019025	Ka ba 'yɛr, 'Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, pie lɛ wʋ tara.'
42019026	Wʋ 'yɛr naa, 'N 'yɛrɛ yɩ naa ɩka nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara wʋn lɛ nyɛn dɔɔl, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba tara ɛ, tɩ tara bɩ̃lãa ban den a bɩ̃lãa ala.
42019027	Tɩchɛ a n dɔ̃dẽme bala na ba bʋɔrɔ ma ɩka n ɩ a ba nãa ɛ, yɩ nyɔɔr ba waan wa kʋ a ka a n niem.' "
42019028	Yesu na 'yɛr a anyãna baar wʋ de ban nie ka ba duoro a Jerusalɛm.
42019029	A lɛ wʋn wa gbʋrɔ a Betefagɩ nɩ a Betanɩ, tɔ̃ɔ ben be ka ba bʋɔlɔ Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ, wʋ tʋ̃ naa a wʋ poturbo ayi tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba.
42019030	"Yɩ chen a tẽbile 'lɔ a yɩ niem, yɩn wa kpɩɛrɛ a tẽe pɔ yɩn nyɛn bʋ̃pɔlbile ban lũ, baa do wʋ jaa sɛrɛ ɛ, yɩ for wʋ waan.
42019031	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ wa sʋʋr yɩ naa, 'Ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ foro a bʋ̃pɔlbile?' Yɩ 'yɛr wʋ, 'A sɩ Soro lɛ bʋɔrɔ wʋ.' "
42019032	A bala wʋn tʋ̃ chen tɩ nyɛ a lɛ nɛ wʋn 'yɛr ba.
42019033	Ban wa foro a bʋ̃pɔlbile, a bʋ̃pɔlbile dẽme sʋʋr ba naa, "Ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ foro a bʋ̃pɔlbile?"
42019034	A ba 'yɛr, "A sɩ Soro lɛ bʋɔrɔ wʋ."
42019035	Ba waan naa a bʋ̃pɔlbile wa kʋ a Yesu, na ba 'yɩɛr a ba fɔɔr dɔɔl a bʋ̃pɔlbile ju, tɩ nyɔɔ a Yesu ka wʋ do jɩ̃nɛ.
42019036	A lɛ wʋn chiine, lɛ mɩ lɛ a nɩbɛ 'yɩɛrɛ a fɔɔr den a sɔr.
42019037	Wʋn chen wa gbʋrɔ a jie a sɔr na suu a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ ju, a nɩyɔɔ bala na turo wʋ piel chɩlɛ nɩ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ na ba pɛɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala a jaa ban nyɛ jũu.
42019038	"Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a nãa 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃! Nyã'maar ben a saaju, ka a tɩɩr be a saaju jaa saaju."
42019039	Ka a Faraseemɩne na be a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ, 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Wiwile tãn a fʋ poturbo a ba bar a gɔ̃n."
42019040	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ala ɩ ba bar a gɔ̃n, kʋsɩbɛ na pɔɔrɔ naa gɔ̃mɔ̃."
42019041	Yesu na wa tara a Jerusalɛm na wʋ nyɛ a tẽe wʋ kõn kʋ wʋ,
42019042	tɩ 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ a fʋ̃ʋ, fʋ̃ʋ gba ta bɔ̃ɔ a bon 'lɔ a dɩna bɩbir nɩ taa waan nyã'maar, tɩchɛ a sɔɔl naa a fʋ sɛ̃.
42019043	A bɩbir na wa vɩɛ yɩ naa, ka a yɩ dɔ̃dẽme wa jilʋ̃ yɩ gʋɔr gʋɔr a jie wʋ jaa.
42019044	Ban nɛb yɩn ŋmɛr nɩ a yɩ bibiir nɩ a yɩ tẽe ba kʋ̃ wa bar kʋsɩr ka wʋ dɔɔl wʋ tɔ ju ɛ, bojũu yaa tɩɛr tɔ a sɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na waara a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ."
42019045	Wʋ pãa tɩ kpɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ na wʋ piel dire a bala na daara bara.
42019046	Na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'A n yir na ɩ naa a puorfʋ jie,' tɩchɛ ka a yɩn maal wʋ a 'nãnyisɩ sɔɔlfʋ jie.' "
42019047	Bɩbir jaa lɛ wʋ wile ba be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir, tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ bʋɔrɔ a wʋ kʋfʋ.
42019048	Tɩchɛ baa bɔ̃ɔ lɛ ban na ɩ ɛ, bojũu nɩbɛ ba jaa 'yɔ̃ɔn toor chɛlɛ a wʋ 'yɛr.
42020001	A bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ Yesu ben a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, wile a nɩbɛ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋrɔ ba. Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ wa a wʋ sɛ̃.
42020002	Na ba sʋʋr wʋ, "'Yɛr kʋ sɩ a jie fʋn nyɛ a sɔr maala nɩ a anyãna, an kʋ fʋ a sɔr nyã?"
42020003	Ka a Yesu mɩ 'yɛr, "N tara na sʋʋrfʋ na sʋʋr yɩ.
42020004	A Jɔɔn na dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ an lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, Nãaŋmɩn lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ bɩɩ nɩrɛ lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ?"
42020005	A ba lɩɛb guor taa 'yɛrɛ, "Ala ɩ sɩ ben 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, wʋn lɩɛb sʋʋr sɩ, ŋmɩnɛ a saa sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ?
42020006	Tɩchɛ sɩn mɩ 'yɛr ɩka nɩrɛ lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, a nɩbɛ ba jaa na lɔb sɩn nɩ kʋsɩbɛ, bojũu ba jaa sɔɔn de ɩka Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ."
42020007	Be lɛ a ba 'yɛr, "Saa bɔ̃ɔ a jie an yi ɛ."
42020008	A Yesu mɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N mɩ kʋ̃ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a jie ɩn nyɛ a sɔr maala nɩ a anyãna ɛ."
42020009	Yesu chɛnɛ na 'yɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛ na wʋ lɔb a sʋkpa nyã kʋ ba, "Daba lɛ bʋr a tɩwɔ̃nsɩ de kʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ a ba kaara, tɩ yɔ chen tɛɛr na wʋ tɩ kor be jaa.
42020010	Ka a tɩɩr wɔ̃mɔ̃ mʋɔfʋ sɔ̃ɔ wa ta ka wʋ ir a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɩ̃sʋɔ tʋ̃ a bala na kaara wʋ a puo ka ba pɔr a wɔ̃mɔ̃ amɩne tɩr. Tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ bala ŋme wʋ bar ka wʋ kul nũjaal.
42020011	Ka wʋ lɛ tʋ̃ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɩ̃sʋɔ go, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ mɩ ba lɛ ŋme ŋme naa tɩ tu tu wʋ bar, ka wʋ mɩ lɩɛb kul a nũjaala.
42020012	Ka wʋ lɛ maal tʋ̃ a ata sʋɔ ka ba ŋme a 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ baal 'mɔɔ lɔb bar a yõo.
42020013	"A puo sʋɔ pãa 'yɛr, 'Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ɩn ɩ? Ɩn tʋ̃n a n bidanʋ̃naa amɩne sɛ̃ ban jo wʋn vĩ.'
42020014	Tɩchɛ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ na wa nyɛ a bidaba na waara a ba guor taa 'yɛr, 'Nyã lɛ ɩ a bʋ̃dire, yɩ ɩ a sɩ kʋ wʋ bar tɩ de a bonsɩ.'
42020015	Na ba nyɔɔ wʋ vu yin a puo kõkoor na ba tɩ kʋ wʋ. Bo lɛ a puo sʋɔ na wa ɩ a nɩbɛ banyãna?
42020016	Wʋn wa kʋ naa a nɩbɛ banyãna bar, tɩ de a puo kʋ nɩyor." Lɛ a nɩbɛ na wa wõ a 'yɛrbir nyã a ba 'yɛr, "A kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a lɛ ɛ."
42020017	Ka a Yesu kaa ba a lɛ a tɩ̃ɩɩ tɩ sʋʋr, "Ala ɩ a kʋ̃ ɩ a lɛ ɛ, a par nɩ bo an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'A kʋsɩr 'lɔ a mɩmɩɛrbɛ na tɔr lɛ ɩ a kʋsɩr ju?'
42020018	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa lo a kʋsɩr nyã ju na kar kara, tɩchɛ 'lɔ mɩ wa lo dib ɩ̃sʋɔ wʋn pʋrpʋr wʋ naa."
42020019	Ka a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ kaara sɔr 'lɔ ban na tu nyɔɔ wʋ fɔɔ, bojũu ba bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka bala lɛ wʋ lɔb a sʋkpa gbɛb, tɩchɛ na ba joro a nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ.
42020020	Ba jʋrɔ naa Yesu, na ba ir nɩbɛ tʋ̃ ka ba tɩ maala fɩka nɩsʋ̃n tɩ jʋrɔ wʋ. Ba bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba wõ a wʋ nɛɛ 'yɛrbie de nyɔɔn wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ kpɛ̃ɔ sʋɔ nũu pɔ, na ɩ a paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ.
42020021	A nɛbɛr nɩbɛ banyãna sʋʋr wʋ naa, "Wiwile sɩ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka fʋ ma 'yɛr naa na fʋ wiil a lɛ na tor, faa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩbɛ gar taa ɛ, tɩchɛ na fʋ wile a nɩbɛ Nãaŋmɩn sɔr nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
42020022	Sɔr ben be a sɩn yab a lõpo kʋ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa bɩɩ sɔr ba be be ɛ?"
42020023	Yesu nyɛn a ba yɛ̃ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba,
42020024	"Yɩ wiil ma a libikur. An ju ŋmaa nɩ a wʋ yuor lɛ be be?"
42020025	A ba 'yɛr, "A Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa lɛ." A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba. "Yɩ kʋ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa a ala na ɩ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa bon na yɩ mɩ de a ala na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bon mɩ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn."
42020026	Ba bɛr wʋn a nɛɛ faa a anyãna wʋn 'yɛr a chãsara, ka nɛɛr 'maa ba nɩ a 'yɛr nyãna wʋn 'yɛr, a ba ɩ gbulo gbulo.
42020027	A Saduseemɩne na 'yɛr ɩka a kũu pɔ irfʋ ba be be ɛ, bamɩne wan a Yesu sɛ̃ wa sʋʋr wʋ.
42020028	"Wiwile, Mosesɩ sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ gãn pɔ kʋ sɩ ɩka, ala ɩ daba kul pɔɔ na wʋ wa kpi, tɩchɛ ka a pɔɔ ba dɔɔ bie ɛ, a yɛbɛ wʋ de a pɔɔ kʋɔr kul na wʋ dɔɔ bie kʋ a yɛbɛ.
42020029	Yɛɛr ayopõi lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be, ka a ba kpɛ̃ɛ kul pɔɔ na wʋ kpi, tɩ baa dɔɔ bie ɛ.
42020030	Ka a wʋ turo
42020031	nɩ a ata sʋɔ mɩ kul a pɔɔ, tɩ kpi, lɛ a yɛɛr ayopõi bala mɩ, kul a pɔɔ tɩ kpi baa dɔɔ bie ɛ.
42020032	A baaraa jaa ka a pɔɔ mɩ kpi.
42020033	An be a lɛ, bala wa ir a kũu pɔ, buor sʋɔ pɔɔ lɛ wʋn ɩ, an ɩ ba jaa ayopõi kul wʋ naa?"
42020034	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩbɛ na be ka a wɛr pɔ, kulo nɩ taa.
42020035	Tɩchɛ a bala na sɛɛn na ir a kũu pɔ a bɩbir 'lɔ, bala ba kulo taa ɛ.
42020036	Bala kʋ̃ lɛ kpi go ɛ, nɩtãa lɛ a malakasɩ na ba kpire ɛ. Ba ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn bibiir an ɩ bala lɛ ɩ a kũu pɔ irfʋ bibiir.
42020037	A kũu pɔ irfʋ, Mosesɩ mɩ wiil sɩ naa ɩka a ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ a lɛ wʋn sɛb a wʋ gãn pɔ, a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛrɛ nɩ wʋ a tɩbile na 'lɩrɛ a bũu, ka wʋ sɛb ɩka Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, Abraham, Isaakɩ nɩ a Jekɔb Nãaŋmɩn.
42020038	Waa ɩ kũn Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ɩn a vʋɛ Nãaŋmɩn a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ ba jaa ɩ vʋɛ."
42020039	Ka a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe bamɩne 'yɛr, "Wiwile, fʋ 'yɛr vɩla."
42020040	Nɩrɛ jaa ba lɛ 'la sʋʋr wʋ go ɛ.
42020041	Yesu pãa sʋʋr ba naa, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a ɩ ka a nɩbɛ 'yɛrɛ ɩka a Kɩrɩsɩto ɩn a Nãa David Bidaba?
42020042	A Nãa David mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr a wʋ yiel gãn pɔ, 'A n Soro Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ a n Soro nyã wʋn ir, "Jɩ̃nɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ jie,
42020043	ka n wa de a fʋ dɔ̃dẽme bin a fʋ gbɛɛ pĩlem." '
42020044	A Nãa David bʋɔl wʋ naa a wʋ Soro, ŋmɩnɛ wʋn lɛ ɩrɛ wa ɩ a wʋ bie?"
42020045	A nɩbɛ na chɛlɛ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ, ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo.
42020046	"Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe 'yɔ̃ɔ. Ba nʋ̃ naa fuu vɛɛsɩ sufʋ, na ba nʋ̃ ɩka ba puoro ba a dar pɔ. A ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yie a niem lɛ ba ma jɩ̃nɛ na ba jɩ̃nɛ a jibɛrɛ jie bala wa lɔ̃ɔ dire.
42020047	Bala lɛ ma fɔlɔ a pɔɔ kɔɛ yie na ba ma sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kor bʋɔrɔ ɩka a nɩbɛ ba kaara ba. Ban nyɛn ge dɛɛr."
42021001	Yesu dʋɔn kaa nyɛ a tara dẽme na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a ba libie be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir.
42021002	Wʋ nyɛn pɔɔ kʋɔr nɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ mɩ na 'yɔ̃ɔ kobsɩ ayi.
42021003	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a pɔɔ kʋɔr nɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ nyã 'yɔ̃ɔn gar ba jaa.
42021004	A nɩbɛ banyãna ma ir 'yɔ̃ɔ tɩ chɛ a libie amɩne, tɩchɛ a pɔɔ nyã bon jaa wʋn tara lɛ wʋ de 'yɔ̃ɔ."
42021005	A Yesu poturbo bamɩne 'yɛrɛ na a lɛ ban maal a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir nɩ a kʋsɩr vɩɛlsɩ, nɩ a kʋfʋsɩ ban kʋ Nãaŋmɩn. Tɩchɛ ka Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba,
42021006	"A kʋsɩbɛ anyãna yɩn nyɛ a kana, sɔ̃ɔ waara naa, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ dɔɔl a wʋ tɔ ju ɛ, a jaa na wɛl gã tẽe."
42021007	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Wiwile, dabor lɛ an ɩ? Bo lɛ na ɩ a jɩ̃nɛ ala wa bʋɔrɔ a ɩfʋ?"
42021008	A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ka nɩrɛ taa bɛl yɩ ɛ. Bojũu nɩyɔɔ lɛ na de a n yuor waan wa 'yɛrɛ ɩka, 'Maa lɛ ba ɩ,' ka a ɩ, 'Sɔ̃ɔ gbʋr naa.' Yɩ taa turo ba ɛ.
42021009	Yɩn wa wõ jɛɛr nɩ faa taa, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ yɩ ɛ. A anyãna lɛ na de nie wa, tɩchɛ a ba ɩ a baarfʋ lɛ ɛ."
42021010	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩbɛ na ir tɩ jɛɛr nɩ a tẽe ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩbɛ, ka a nãmɩne mɩ ir jɛɛrɛ taa.
42021011	A tẽe na mɩr naa a jie wʋ jaa ka a kɔ̃ lo ka a baal dɛbɛ de jiir a jaa ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ nɩ jɩ̃nɛ yi saaju.
42021012	"Sɛrɛ tɩchɛ ka anyãna na wa ɩ ban ge yɩ naa, na ba nyɔɔr yɩ chiin a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir na ba fɩr yɩ chiin tɩ pɔɔ. Ban fɩr yɩn chiin a nãmɩne yie nɩ a paal nɩbɛrɛ jie a n yuor jũu.
42021013	A anyãna na kʋ yɩn sɔr ka yɩ di a n dãasɩɛ kʋ ba.
42021014	Tɩchɛ yɩ ta ɩ ka a ɩ yɩ tɩɛrɛ a lɛ yɩn na tɩ 'yɛr faa yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
42021015	Bojũu maa lɛ na kʋ yɩ a 'yɛr nɩ a yɛ̃ ka a yɩ sãma dẽme kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ jie chɩɩr yɩ ɛ.
42021016	A yɩ sãamɩne nɩ a yɩ mamɩne, yɛɛr nɩ a yɩ bal nɩbɛ nɩ a yɩ barmɩne na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ ka ba kʋ a yɩ bamɩne.
42021017	Nɩbɛ ba jaa na 'laar yɩ naa a maa jũu.
42021018	Tɩchɛ a yɩ jukɔɔlbir kʋ̃ wa wɛ ɛ.
42021019	Yɩn chɛnɛ sɔɔ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ yɩn faan yɩ mɩ̃ɛ.
42021020	"Yɩn wa nyɛ a sojasɩ a ba wa ŋmaa jilʋ̃ a Jerusalɛm, yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a wʋ wɛlfʋ gbʋr jaa yɛ̃yɛ̃.
42021021	Ka a bala na pãa be a Judiya ba joro duoro a tɔ̃n jur. A bala mɩ na be a a Jerusalɛm tẽe pɔ, yɩ joro yire, ka a bala mɩ na be a tẽe kõkoor ba ta lɛ kpɛ a tẽe pɔ go ɛ.
42021022	A sɔ̃ɔ nyãna lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na kpãa a Isɩral nɩbɛ, a kpãafʋ nyã na ɩn a lɛ ban sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ.
42021023	A bɩbir nyã na ɩn wõm kʋ a pɔɔ pʋʋr nɩ a bipɩlɛ dẽme, dɔɔyɛ kpɛ̃ɛ na ben a wɛr pɔ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn suur lɛ dire a wʋ nɩbɛ.
42021024	Sɔkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ ban kʋn ba, tɩ nyɔɔr ba nɩpɔɔrsɩ kaar kʋ a paalsɩ. Ka a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ na nɛɛrɛ naa a Jerusalɛm wa tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɔ̃ɔ kʋ ba.
42021025	"Yɩn nyɛn jɩ̃nsɩ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ pɔ, ŋmɛra pɔ nɩ a ŋmɛrbie pɔ. Tuo na pɔɔn nɩbʋrɔ jaa na be ka wɛr ju, ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a nɩbɛ, a man kpɛ̃ɛ kʋ̃ɔ na kara na a ɔɔrɔ.
42021026	Dãbɩ̃ɛ nyã na vɛ̃ naa ka a nɩbɛ pɛl, bojũu ba bɔ̃ɔn naa a dɔɔyɛ nyã na waara a wɛr pɔ, a saaju bomo a jaa na dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ naa.
42021027	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ban nyɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na yi a julõjuur pɔ, waara nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ a tɩɩr kpɛ̃ɛ.
42021028	A yele anyãna wa ɩrɛ, yɩ ir ara tɩ jɛɛr a yɩ jur, bojũu a yɩ faafʋ gbʋrɔ naa."
42021029	Sʋkpa nyã lɛ a Yesu lɔb kʋ ba, na wa 'yɛr, "Yɩ kaa a pɔlpɔl tɩɛ nɩ a tɩɩr a jaa.
42021030	Yɩn wa nyɛ ka a tʋɔrɔ a vaar yɩ ma bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka tʋl tara naa.
42021031	A lɛ mɩ lɛ, yɩn wa nyɛ a yelsɩ anyãna ka a ɩrɛ, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ gbʋr naa.
42021032	"Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka nɩsaal jaa kʋ̃ kpi baar ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a yelsɩ anyãna ɩ ɛ.
42021033	A saaju nɩ a tẽe, a jaa na wa baaraa, tɩchɛ a maa 'yɛrbie kʋ̃ wa baar ɛ.
42021034	"Yɩ guro yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, ka a yɩ nyãa taa pɔɔ ɛ, nɩ dãa kuolfʋ nɩ a ɩ̃gãn nyã bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ ka a bɩbir nyã taa wa dũu yɩ fɩka chɛbaa na tɛb ɛ.
42021035	Bojũu a lɛ na ɩ ɩn na wa, pɔɔn nɩrɛ jaa na be ka a wɛr nyã pɔ.
42021036	Yɩ kaara na yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn, na yɩ tʋ̃ɔ jo yi a ala a jaa na wa wa ɩ pɔ, na yɩn tʋ̃ɔ ara a maa Nɩsaal Bie niem."
42021037	A Yesu ma wile naa a nɩbɛ be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir, tɩchɛ ka a tɩ̃sɔɔ ka wʋ ma do a tɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ tɩ gã a be.
42021038	Ka a nɩbɛ ma chɛnɛ ŋmaa ir a bibio wa be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ɩka ba wa chɛl a wʋ 'yɛr.
42022001	A Paanʋ̃kõo Lɔ̃ɔfʋ ban bʋɔlɔ a Gõl Bar Difʋ gbʋrɔ naa.
42022002	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe bʋɔrɔ sɔr 'lɔ ban na tu nyɔɔ a Yesu jaa jom, bojũu ba joro naa a nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ.
42022003	Ka a Satan pãa kpɛ a Judas na yi a Isɩkariyot na ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ pie nɩ ayi ɩ̃sʋɔ.
42022004	Wʋ ir chen a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir gugurbo sɛ̃, ka ba tɩ man taa lɛ wʋn na ɩ, ka ba nyɔɔ a Yesu.
42022005	Ba pʋɔ pɛl naa ka ba sɔɔ ɩka ban kʋ wʋ naa libie.
42022006	Judas sɔɔ naa na wʋ kaara bʋɔrɔ sɔr 'lɔ wʋn na nyɔɔ a Yesu kʋ ba ka a nɩyɔɔ ba be be ɛ.
42022007	A Paanʋ̃kõo bɩbir vɩɛ naa, ka ban kʋ a Gõl Bar Difʋ pɛr.
42022008	Yesu tʋ̃n a Pita nɩ Jɔɔn na wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ chen tɩ chɔɔr jie ka sɩ chen tɩ di a Gõl Bar Difʋ."
42022009	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ chen tɩ chɔɔr?"
42022010	A wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩn wa tɩ kpɛ a tẽe pɔ, yɩn tuor daba na tuo kʋ̃ɔ nɩ yuor yɩ turo wʋ tɩ kpɛ̃n a yir 'lɔ pɔ wʋn kpɛ.
42022011	Na yɩ tɩ 'yɛr a yir sʋɔ, a wiwile lɛ 'yɛr ɩka sɩ wa sʋʋr fʋ kaa, ka nyɩnɛ lɛ a sãanba die be, ka 'lɔ naa wʋ poturbo na wa di a Gõl Bar Difʋ?
42022012	Wʋn wiil yɩn bɔɔpɩɛ dikpɛ̃ɛ ban chɔɔr yɩ maal a bʋ̃diir a be."
42022013	Ba chen tɩ nyɛ a lɛ nɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr na ba chɔɔr a bʋ̃diir a be.
42022014	A sɔ̃ɔ na wa ta Yesu nɩ a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nsɩ wa jɩ̃nɛ naa a bʋ̃diir par.
42022015	Be lɛ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N bʋɔrɔ na yɔɔ jaa ɩka n 'mataa din yɩ a Gõl Bar nyã bʋ̃diir tɩ na n di a dɔɔyɛ.
42022016	Bojũu n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka n kʋ̃ lɛ di yaa go ɛ, wa tɩ tãn yele jaa na maal baar a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
42022017	Wʋn wa de a dãa naa ŋmele wʋ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nsɩ, "Yɩ de a anyã nyũ lʋɔr taa.
42022018	Bojũu n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka n kʋ̃ lɛ nyũ a dãa anyãna go ɛ, tɩ tãn a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ waa daar."
42022019	Wʋ lɛ den a paanʋ̃ɔ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan tɩ na wʋ ŋma de kʋ ba tɩ 'yɛr, "A maa ɩ̃gãn lɛ a nyãna ɩn diere kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ maala a nɩtɔ̃ tɩɛrɛ nɩ ma."
42022020	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ ban wa di baar wʋ den a ŋmele tɩ 'yɛr, "A ŋmele nyã ɩn a nɛtɩr paalaa na ɩ a maa jɩ̃ɩ na kpaar a yɩ jũu.
42022021	"Tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na garʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ma lɛ n 'mataa dire nɩ a bʋ̃diir.
42022022	A maa Nɩsaal Bie na chen naa nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bin, tɩchɛ nɛbier ben a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na garʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ma."
42022023	A ba piel sʋrɔ taa ɩka a ba buor sʋɔ lɛ na pãa tʋ̃ a nɩtɔ̃.
42022024	Ka nɛchɩrɛ mɩ ir a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ pɔ, a ba chɩrɛ taa bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bɔ̃ɔ buor sʋɔ lɛ na ɩ a ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ.
42022025	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãmɩne ɛ, ma fɩrɛ naa a nɩbɛ, ka a bala mɩ na wile a ba kpɩ̃ɛn bʋɔlɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ, nɩsʋ̃nbɔ.
42022026	Tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ a ba ɩ lɛ lɛ ɛ, a 'lɔ na ɩ a yɩ kpɛ̃ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ na ɩ a yɩ jaa bibile, a 'lɔ na kaara yɩ, 'lɔ lɛ na tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ yɩ.
42022027	Nɩbuor sʋɔ lɛ ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ, a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a bʋ̃diir par, bɩɩ a 'lɔ na põnõ? A ba ɩ a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a bʋ̃diir par ɛ? Tɩchɛ a maa na ɩ a yɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ben a yɩ sɛ̃, ɩ a yɩ bʋ̃ põnõ.
42022028	"Yɩn lɛ ɩ a nɩbɛ bala na chɛnɛ ara gu ma a n wõm pɔ.
42022029	N kʋ yɩn a nãalʋ̃ʋ nɩtãa lɛ a n Sãa na kʋ ma a nãalʋ̃ʋ.
42022030	Ka maa nɩ yɩn lɔ̃ɔ di tɩ nyũ be a n nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ, na yɩ jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju tɔɔrɔ a Isɩral balsɩ pie nɩ ayi 'yɛr.
42022031	"Simon, Simon, a Satan sʋɔr sɔr Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɩka wʋ yɩɛl yɩ chi kaar.
42022032	Tɩchɛ a fʋ̃ʋ Pita n sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ fʋ ɩka, a fʋ sɔɔfʋ ta bʋ̃bʋr ɛ, a fʋ̃ʋ wa lɩɛb puor, fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a fʋ taaba ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn."
42022033	Tɩchɛ ka a Simon 'yɛr, "N Soro, n chɔɔr naa ɩka maa nɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ na lɔ̃ɔ kpɛ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, na sɩ 'mataa kpi."
42022034	A Yesu 'yɛr, "A fʋ̃ʋ Pita, sɛrɛ ka a nɔraa kõ a dɩna fʋn chɩɩr gbɛɛ ata ɩka faa bɔ̃ɔ ma ɛ."
42022035	Be lɛ a Yesu pãa sʋʋr ba, "Ɩn dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃ yɩ a nũjaala, yaa tara libie ɛ, bɩɩ wʋɔ nɩ nafɔɔr ɛ, yɩ dɔ̃ɔ bɔ bon faa bɩɩ?" A ba 'yɛr ɩka baa bɔ bon jaa faa ɛ.
42022036	A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, fʋ̃ʋ nyã na tara libie de, fʋ̃ʋ nyã mɩ na tara wʋɔ de, fʋ̃ʋ nyã na ba wa tara sɔkpɛ̃ɛ ɛ, de a fʋ fuu da na fʋ dãn a sɔkpɛ̃ɛ.
42022037	A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'Ba sɔr wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ a tʋ̃dɛbɛ dẽme pɔ.' N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka maa lɛ ban maal a lɛ nɛ, ɔ̃ɔ, a lɛ ban sɛb a n yele a gbʋrɔ na tafʋ."
42022038	Ka a poturbo 'yɛr, "Sɩ Soro nyɛ sɔbɛrɛ ayi." A wʋ 'yɛr, "A sɛɛ naa."
42022039	Yesu yin duoro a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ ju, nɩtãa lɛ wʋn ma ɩrɛ ka a wʋ poturbo turo wʋ.
42022040	Wʋn wa ta a jie wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn na yɩ taa lo a bɛɛr kaa pɔ ɛ."
42022041	Wʋ tɔɔn jãa ba bɩ̃lãa fɩka kʋsɩr fʋn na lɔb ka wʋ ta, na wʋ gbʋr dumo sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ,
42022042	"N Sãa, ala ɩ fʋ bʋɔrɔ naa, de a dɔɔyɛ ŋmele nyãna bar ma, a ɩ a fʋ bɔfʋ a ta ɩ a maa bɔfʋ ɛ."
42022043	Be lɛ a malaka yi be a saaju wa a wʋ sɛ̃ wa 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ.
42022044	A nɩbaal na kpɛ wʋ a lɛ, ka wʋ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ jaa ka a nyĩe hãna wʋ loro tẽe fɩka jɩ̃ɩ.
42022045	Wʋn wa ir a Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jie lɩɛb chen tɩ nyɛ ka a wʋ poturbo gã gur nɩ pʋsɔ̃ɔ.
42022046	Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ gã guro? Yɩ ir sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn na yɩ taa lo a bɛɛr kaa pɔ ɛ."
42022047	Wʋn chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ a lɛ ka a ɩ a nɩyɔɔ daan sãa, ka a 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Judas a Pie Nɩ Ayi ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ de ba a nie. Wʋ tɔɔn ta a Yesu puor wʋ.
42022048	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Judas, fʋ ben de puorfʋ garʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a maa Nɩsaal Bie?"
42022049	Yesu poturbo na nyɛ a lɛ na ɩrɛ ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Sɩ Soro, sɩ chɩɛrɛ nɩ a sɔbɛrɛ bɩɩ?"
42022050	Ka a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ chɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ gbãgbaa nũsʋ̃ɔ toor ŋmaa.
42022051	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩ ta lɛ maal a lɛ ɛ." Tɩ na wʋ sɩɩr a daba toor ka wʋ choo.
42022052	A Yesu pãa sʋʋr a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir gugurbo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nɩdierbe, "A mɔ̃ nɩbier lɛ n ɩ ka yɩ waan sɔbɛrɛ nɩ dakʋrsɩ a n nyɔɔfʋ jie bɩɩ?
42022053	Maa nɩ yɩn lɛ be be bɩbir jaa be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, yaa nyɔɔ ma ɛ, tɩchɛ a yɩ bɩbir vɩɛ naa ka a libe mɩ di nãa."
42022054	Ba nyɔɔ naa Yesu, na ba chiine a bɔɔrlo nãa yir, ka a Pita mɩ be a puor na wʋ turo.
42022055	Ban tɩ ta ba gbɔɔn bũu be a bɛchaar sãlsɔɔ 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ ka a Pita mɩ tɩ pʋɔ ba ka ba 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ.
42022056	Ka a gbãgbapɔɔbile nyɛ wʋ a bũu na chaar na wʋ kaara wʋ jaa tɩ̃ɩɩ tɩ wa 'yɛr, "A daba nyã mɩ ɩn a wʋ poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ."
42022057	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita chiir 'yɛr, "Pɔɔ, n ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ."
42022058	A ba kor ɛ ka a nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ nyɛ wʋ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Fʋ mɩ ɩn a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ." Ka a Pita 'yɛr, "Daba, n ba ɩ a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ."
42022059	A ba lɛ kor ɛ, ka a nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr, "A ba ɩ baal ɛ, a daba nyã ɩn a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ bojũu Galilee lɛ wʋ yi."
42022060	Ka a Pita 'yɛr, "Daba, n ba bɔ̃ɔ a ala fʋn 'yɛrɛ ɛ." Ka a nɔraa mɩ tɔ̃ɔ kõ a lɛ nɛ.
42022061	Ka a Yesu lɩɛb na wʋ kaa a Pita, a wʋ tɔ̃ɔ tɩɛr tɔ a lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ɩka, "Sɛrɛ tɩchɛ ka a nɔraa kõ a dɩna fʋn chiir man gbɛɛ ata."
42022062	Ka a Pita ir yi a yõo na wʋ tɩ kõ nɩbaal kõn.
42022063	A dɔɔr bala na nyɔɔ a Yesu, piel na ba ɩrɛ wʋ laara tɩ ŋmiere wʋ.
42022064	Ba pɔɔ wʋ naa nɩbie tɩ sʋʋr, "Bɔ̃ɔ na fʋ 'yɛr kʋ sɩ a nɩnyɩnɛ na ŋme fʋ?"
42022065	Ba lɛ den 'yɛrbidɛbɛ yɔɔ tʋ tʋn wʋ.
42022066	A wɛr na wa chaar, a Juu nɩbɛ nɩdierbe nɩ a ba bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ, nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe lɔ̃ɔn taa, ka ba tara a Yesu waan a be.
42022067	A ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ, 'yɛr kʋ sɩ." Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Maa 'yɛr, yɩ kʋ̃ sɔɔ ɛ.
42022068	Ala ɩ n sʋʋr yɩn 'yɛr yɩ kʋ̃ haa ma nɛɛ ɛ.
42022069	Tɩchɛ an yi a dɩna chiine, a maa Nɩsaal Bie na jɩ̃nɛ naa Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ sɔɔ nũsʋ̃ɔ jie."
42022070	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie ɔ?" Kaa a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩn lɛ 'yɛr ɩka lɛ n ɩ."
42022071	Ka ba pãa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ sɩ lɛ bʋɔrɔ dãasɩɛ go? Sɩ wõn yi a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɛɛ pɔ."
42023001	Be lɛ a nɩyɔɔ bala pãa tara a Yesu chiin a be a paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ Pilate sɛ̃.
42023002	Na ba tɩ piel 'yɛrɛ a 'yɛrsɩ anyãna dɔɔlɔ wʋ, "Sɩ nyɛn a daba nyãna ka wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nɩbɛ 'yɛr, a ba ta yab a lõpo kʋ a Nãa Siisa ɛ, na wʋ lɛ 'yɛr ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa na ɩ a nãa."
42023003	Ka a Pilate sʋʋr a Yesu, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa ɔ?" Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, fʋ̃ʋ baa 'yɛr."
42023004	Ka a Pilate pãa 'yɛr kʋ a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛ, "N ba nyɛ chɛfʋ jaa a daba nyã jie ɛ."
42023005	Tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ tɔr tɩ chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ, "Wiilfʋ nyãna lɛ wʋ tara dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a nɩbɛ be a Judiya. Galilee lɛ wʋ piel a yele nyãna be wa tãn a ka."
42023006	Pilate na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ ka wʋ sʋrɔ, Galilee lɛ a daba yi bɩɩ?
42023007	Wʋn wa bɔ̃ɔn ka a Hɛrɔd paal nɩrɛ lɛ, wʋ vɛ̃ naa ka ba tara wʋ chiin tɩ kʋ a Hɛrɔd, ka ɩ a Jerusalɛm lɛ wʋ mɩ be a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
42023008	Hɛrɔd na wa nyɛ a Yesu, wʋ pʋɔ pɛl naa, bojũu a kor wʋn wõ a Yesu yele na wʋ bʋɔrɔ a wʋ nyɛfʋ, ka wʋ tʋ̃ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃.
42023009	Na wʋ sʋʋr a Yesu sʋʋr yɔɔ tɩ waa haa wʋ nɛɛ ɛ.
42023010	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe na ara a be 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr kpɩ̃ɛn dɔɔlɔ wʋ.
42023011	Hɛrɔd nɩ a wʋ sojasɩ maal a Yesu dɛɛr na ba ɩrɛ wʋ laara. Ba su wʋ naa a nãa fuu tɩ lɩɛb wʋ chiin a Pilate sɛ̃.
42023012	Hɛrɔd nɩ a Pilate dɔ̃ɔ tara taa nɩ 'yɛr, tɩ a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ba maal a 'yɛr.
42023013	Be lɛ a Pilate bʋɔl a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ, nɩ a tẽe nɩbɛrɛ, nɩ a nɩbɛ ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa.
