42023014	Na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn lɛ waan a daba nyãna a n sɛ̃ wa 'yɛr ɩka wʋ sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ naa a nɩbɛ. N vɩɛr naa a wʋ 'yɛr a yɩ jaa niem ka a ala yɩn 'yɛr dɔɔl wʋ ba ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
42023015	Hɛrɔd mɩ ba nyɛ yele jaa a wʋ jie ɛ, ala lɛ so ka wʋ lɛ lɩɛb wʋ wa kʋ sɩ, yɩn mɩ̃ɛ nyɛ naa wʋn ba maal yele jaa na sɛɛn kũu ɛ.
42023016	A lɛ jũu ɩn vɛ̃ naa ka ba fɔb wʋ tɩchɛ kaa n bar wʋ."
42023018	Ka ba jaa ŋme chɛl daa 'yɛrɛ, "Ŋmaa daba nyã ju tɩ na fʋ yuo a Barabasɩ na fʋ kʋ sɩ."
42023019	Ba pɔɔ naa a Barabasɩ, bojũu 'yɛr dɔ̃ɔ lo be a tẽe pɔ, ka wʋ kʋ nɩrɛ.
42023020	Pilate na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ bar a Yesu wʋ lɛ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ go.
42023021	Tɩchɛ ka ba chɛnɛ ŋmiere a chɛlsɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Kpa wʋ a daa ju, kpa wʋ a daa ju."
42023022	Gbɛɛ ata lɛ wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Bo? Bãa dɛɛr lɛ wʋ ɩ? Maa ba nyɛ dɛɛr jaa wʋn sɛɛn kũu ɛ. A lɛ jũu ɩn vɛ̃n ka ba fɔb wʋ tɩ bar wʋ."
42023023	Tɩchɛ ka ba chɛnɛ tãna bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ kpa wʋ a daa ju, ka a ba gɔ̃mɔ̃ wa tʋ̃ɔ wʋ.
42023024	Lɛ lɛ a Pilate 'yɛr ɩka wʋn ɩ naa a lɛ ban 'yɛr.
42023025	A Barabasɩ 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ dam a tẽe na wʋ kʋn nɩrɛ ka ba nyɔɔ wʋ pɔɔ, wʋ yuo wʋn bar tɩ kʋ ba a Yesu.
42023026	A lɛ ban chiine a Yesu, ba nyɔɔn daba yuor na di Simon, Sirenɩ lɛ wʋ yi na wʋ yi a yõo tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a tẽe pɔ. Ba fɩr wʋn de a Yesu daa tuo wʋ ka wʋ turo nɩ wʋ.
42023027	Nɩyɔɔ turo wʋ naa lɔ̃ɔn pɔbɔ, bala lɛ kõnõ waala kʋrɔ wʋ.
42023028	Ka a Yesu lɩɛb 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Jerusalɛm pɔɔbil, yɩ ta kõnõ kʋrɔ ma ɛ, yɩ kõnõ kʋrɔ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a yɩ bibiir.
42023029	Bojũu bɩbir kɔ̃ɔ na wa vɩɛ naa ka yɩ 'yɛr, 'Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a pɔbɔ bala na ab nɩ pɔɔ 'lɔ jaa na ba dɔɔ bie ɛ, bɩɩ bɩrɛ ala jaa na ba 'yɛn kaa ɛ.'
42023030	'A ban pãa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a tɔ̃bɛrɛ, "Yɩ lo pɔɔ sɩ, na yɩ ũu sɩ." '
42023031	Ala ɩ nɩbɛ maala naa a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ a tɩɛ na chɛnɛ ɩ a 'maar, ŋmɩnɛ ban ɩ wʋ 'lɔ wa ko?"
42023032	Dɔɔr ayi na maal dɛɛr, ka ba nyɔɔr ba 'matãan a Yesu chiine a kʋfʋ jie.
42023033	Ba chiin ban tɩ tãn a jie ban bʋɔlɔ Julaa, be lɛ ba kpa ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa a wʋ daa ju, ka a nɩdɛbɛ ayi bala ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ be a Yesu nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, tɩchɛ ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ be a wʋ gʋbaa jie.
42023034	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr, "N Sãa, vɛ̃ kʋ ba, baa bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ ban ɩrɛ ɛ." Gbãm lɛ ba gba na ba põn a wʋ fuusɩ.
42023035	Ka a nɩbɛ ara kaara wʋ, ka a Juu nɩbɛ nɩbɛrɛ ara kpɛrɛ wʋ na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Wʋ ma faan bamɩne, vɛ̃ a wʋ faa a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ala ɩ 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na ir."
42023036	Ka a sojasɩ mɩ wa ɩrɛ wʋ laara, na ba de a dãmiir kʋ wʋ.
42023037	Tɩ na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa, faa a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ."
42023038	Ba sɛb sɛbie mar be a wʋ ju pɔ ka a 'yɛr, "Nyãna lɛ ɩ a Juu Nɩbɛ Nãa".
42023039	A nɩdɛbɛ bala ban lɔ̃ɔ kpan wʋ, ɩ̃sʋɔ tʋrɔ wʋn 'yɛrɛ, "A ba ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa ɛ? Faa a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩ mɩ faa sɩ."
42023040	Tɩchɛ ka a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ 'lɔ gɔ̃nɔ̃ wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Faa joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, an ɩ a kũu 'lɔ lɛ fʋ mɩ kpire.
42023041	Sɩn gefʋ sɛɛn sɩ naa, sɩ nyɛn a lɛ na sɛɛ sɩn maal, tɩchɛ a daba nyã 'lɔ ba maal dɛɛr jaa ɛ."
42023042	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Tɩɛr tɔ ma fʋ̃ʋ wa kpɛ a fu nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
42023043	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, dɩna maa nɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tẽvɩla pɔ."
42023044	A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ dɔ̃ɔ gbʋrɔ a garju sãlsɔɔ tɩchɛ ka a chãa ɩ jaa gbɛb, ka a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ wa tɩ vɩr.
42023045	A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ ba lɛ chaar go ɛ, ka a fɔbaa 'lɔ ban lũ var a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir die pɔ 'mar ayi.
42023046	Be lɛ a Yesu tãn kpɛ̃ɔ jaa 'yɛr, "N Sãa, fʋ nũu pɔ lɛ n de a n sɩɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ." Wʋn wa 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ baar, tɩ vʋʋr a wʋ vʋʋr baaraa.
42023047	A sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na nyɛ a lɛ na ɩ wʋ dãn Nãaŋmɩn tɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ jaa a daba nyã ɩn nɩtor."
42023048	Ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa na lɔ̃ɔ taa a be nyɛn a lɛ na ɩ ka ba lɩɛb pʋsɔ̃ɔ, na ba waala kulo.
42023049	Tɩchɛ a wʋ nɩbɔ̃ɔnsɩ pʋɔn a pɔbɔ bala na tu wʋ yi a Galilee ara tɛɛr tɩ kaara a lɛ na ɩrɛ.
42023050	Daba ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ ben be ban bʋɔlɔ Josefʋ, wʋ pʋɔ naa a nɩbɛrɛ pɔ, na wʋ ɩ nɩsʋ̃ nɩ nɩtor.
42023051	Wʋ tɔr naa a lɛ ban 'yɛr nɩ a lɛ ban ɩrɛ. Wʋ yi naa a Judiya paal pɔ tẽe ban bʋɔlɔ Arimatɩya, wʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ chɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ.
42023052	'Lɔ lɛ chen a Pilate sɛ̃ tɩ sʋɔr a Yesu ɩ̃gãn ɩka wʋ ũu.
42023053	Na wʋ pãa yɔɔ a kũu suun tɩ vil wʋ a fɔpɩla pɔɔ tɩ ũu wʋ a yaa ban chɩ kʋsɩr pɔ, ban ba ũu nɩrɛ sɛrɛ ɛ.
42023054	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ba mɩ chɔɔrɔ ka a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir na piel.
42023055	A pɔbɔ bala nɩ a Yesu na 'mataa yi a Galilee wa, ba tu naa a Josefʋ tɩ nyɛ a yaa nɩ a lɛ ban ũu a Yesu.
42023056	Tɩ na ba pãa lɩɛb kul tɩ chɔɔr a tɩ̃ɩ nɩ a kãnyũu vɩla na tɩ fɔ a Yesu ɩ̃gãn, tɩchɛ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir jũu, baa dam ɛ, ba pɛ̃n naa a lɛ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ na 'yɛr.
42024001	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir divɩɛ bio bibio, a pɔbɔ den a kãnyũur vɩla ala ban chɔɔr chiin a be a yaa par.
42024002	Ba tɩ nyɛn ka a kʋsɩr bil yi a yaa nɛɛ pɔ.
42024003	Ka ba kpɛ tɩchɛ baa nyɛ a Yesu ɩ̃gãn ɛ.
42024004	A ba ara bẽne a lɛ nɛ ka a dɔɔr ayi wa dũu ba ka a ba bʋ̃sursɩ pɛl saa nyɩɩrfʋ kaar.
42024005	Ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a pɔbɔ, ka ba kpa kpa jur a tẽe, tɩchɛ ka a dɔɔr sʋʋr ba, "Bo so ka yɩ bʋɔrɔ a vʋr a kũusɩ pɔ?
42024006	Waa be ka ɛ. Wʋ ir naa. Yɩ tɩɛr a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn be a yɩ sɛ̃, be a Galilee.
42024007	'Ban nyɔɔ naa a maa Nɩsaal Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɩdɛbɛ nuur pɔ, ka ba kʋ ma a daa ju, tɩchɛ a ber ata daar, ka n lɛ ir ɩ vʋr.' "
42024008	Be lɛ ba pãa tɩɛr tɔ a wʋ 'yɛrbie.
42024009	Ban wa yi a yaa par kul, ba tɩ man a anyãna kʋ a Pie Nɩ Bʋ̃'yen nɩ nɩrɛ jaa.
42024010	Mɛɛr na yi Magdala, nɩ Joana nɩ a Jemesɩ ma Mɛɛr nɩ a bamɩne na pʋɔ ba lɛ man a anyãna kʋ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ.
42024011	Tɩchɛ baa sɔɔ de a pɔbɔ 'yɛr ɛ, bojũu a ba 'yɛr nyɛntãan jire.
42024012	An be a lɛ ka Pita vaa ir jo chen a yaa par, na wʋ tɩ guun muul kaa na wʋ nyɛ a fɔpɩla na for gã wʋ yõ, ka wʋ lɩɛb yi tɩ bẽne a lɛ na ɩ.
42024013	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a wʋ poturbo ayi chiine naa a tẽbile ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Emayusɩ na ba jãan a Jerusalɛm ɛ.
42024014	Ka ba pãa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa a lɛ jaa na ɩ.
42024015	A lɛ ban 'yɛrɛ na ba mana a anyãna kʋrɔ taa, ka a Yesu mɩ̃ɛ wa pʋɔ ba a ba 'mataa chiine.
42024016	Tɩchɛ ka a lɩɩ ba a baa bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ.
42024017	Ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Bo lɛ yɩ chiine mana kʋrɔ taa a lɛ mɔ̃?" Ka a nɩbaal kpɛ ba a ba tɛɛ ara.
42024018	Ka ba ɩ̃sʋɔ yuor na di Kɩleopasɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ tɛɛ lɛ ɩ sãan be a Jerusalɛm na faa bɔ̃ɔ lɛ na ɩ a be a ber ayi anyãna ɛ?"
42024019	A wʋ sʋʋr, "Bo yele?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "A Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ, Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ, ka a wʋ 'yɛr nɩ a wʋ maalfʋ kpɛ̃mɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a nɩbɛ niem.
42024020	A bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a sɩ nɩbɛrɛ nyɔɔ wʋn tɩr ɩka ba kʋ, ka ba kpa wʋ a daa ju.
42024021	Tɩchɛ 'lɔ lɛ sɩn mɩ tɩɛrɛ ɩka wʋn faan a Isɩral nɩbɛ. A ala na ɩ dɛɛr jaa nɩ nyã, ber ata nɩ nyã a lɛ na ɩ.
42024022	A sɩ pɔbɔ bamɩne lɛ wa 'maa sɩ nɛɛ, a bibio nyãna lɛ ba chen a yaa par,
42024023	tɩchɛ baa tɩ nyɛ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn ɛ. Na ba wa 'yɛr kʋ sɩ ɩka ba nyɛn malakasɩ ka ba 'yɛr ɩka wʋ ir ɩ vʋr.
42024024	Ka a sɩ taaba bamɩne pãa mɩ chen a yaa par tɩ nyɛ ka ɩ a lɛ nɛ a pɔbɔ na 'yɛr lɛ, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ mɩ̃ɛ baa nyɛ wʋ ɛ."
42024025	Ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yɩ faa tɩɛr lɛ, na yaa tʋ̃ɔ tɩɛr tɔ na yɩ sɔɔ de a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na 'yɛr ɛ?
42024026	A ba ɩ a Nɩ-iraa na din a dɔɔyɛ anyãna tɩ na wʋ pãa kpɛ a wʋ tɩɩr pɔ ɛ?"
42024027	Wʋ piel naa Mosesɩ nɩ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ba jaa, na wʋ pãa wiil ba a par a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr.
42024028	A lɛ ban wa tara a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ ban chiine, a Yesu po naa fɩka tɛɛr wʋn chiine.
42024029	Tɩchɛ ka ba sʋɔr wʋ yãayãabɩlɛ 'yɛrɛ, "Lɩɛb kpɛ wa gã a sɩ sɛ̃, bojũu mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ 'mʋr baar." Ka wʋ lɩɛb kpɛ na gã a ba sɛ̃.
42024030	Be lɛ a ba tɩ 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ a bʋ̃diir par na di, ka wʋ de a paanʋ̃ɔ na puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, tɩ piel ŋmara põnõ ba.
42024031	Ka a ba nɩbie pãa yuo, ka ba bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Yesu lɛ, tɩ wʋ bɔr a ba niem.
42024032	Ka ba 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Ala lɛ so wʋn 'yɛrɛ nɩ sɩ a sɔr pɔ ka a nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ sɩ a lɛ, wʋn wiil sɩ a lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ."
42024033	Be lɛ ba vaa ir fɔɔ jaa lɩɛb chen a Jerusalɛm tɩ nyɛ a Pie Nɩ Bʋ̃'yen nɩ a Yesu poturbo bamɩne na lɔ̃ɔ taa.
42024034	Na ba 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ a sɩ Soro ir ɩ vʋr, na wʋ ir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ wiil a Simon."
42024035	A ba ayi bala pãa man a lɛ na ɩ a sɔr pɔ nɩ a lɛ ban de bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Yesu lɛ wʋn wa ŋma a paanʋ̃ɔ.
42024036	A anyãna ban chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ ka a Yesu mɩ̃ɛ wa ara a ba sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nyã'maar wʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃."
42024037	Ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba a ba mii a lɛ a gbɛ gbɛ, tɩɛr ɩka kpĩin lɛ ba nyɛ.
42024038	A wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Bo lɛ so ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ yɩ a lɛ, a nɩ bo lɛ so ka yɩ baala a lɛ?
42024039	Yɩ kaa nyɛ a n nuur nɩ a gbɛɛ, maa mɩ̃ɛ lɛ, yɩ sɩɩr ma kaa, kpĩin ba lɛ ɛ. Kpĩin maa tara ɩ̃gãn nʋ̃n nɩ kɔɔr nɩtãa lɛ yɩn nyɛ ma ɩn tara ɛ."
42024040	Wʋn 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ baar, wʋ wiil ban a wʋ nuur nɩ a wʋ gbɛɛ.
42024041	Tɩchɛ baa chɛnɛ sɔɔ de sɛrɛ ɛ, nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ba naa ka a nɛɛr 'maa ba, ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Yaa tara bon na kʋ ma ka n di ɛ?"
42024042	Be lɛ ba kʋ wʋ jɩ̃ŋmaa ban wɔ̃,
42024043	ka wʋ 'wɔb be a ba niem.
42024044	Wʋ pãa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A anyãna lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ chɛnɛ be a yɩ sɛ̃. Yele a jaa na sɛb a Mosesɩ nɛɛ pɔ, nɩ a ala na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ gãn pɔ, nɩ a yiel gãn pɔ, a n jũu na ɩ naa lɛ."
42024045	Be lɛ wʋ pãa yuo a ba tɩɛr ka ba tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ala na sɛb a wʋ gãn pɔ.
42024046	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A anyãna lɛ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, a Nɩ-iraa na din dɔɔyɛ na wʋ kpi na wʋ lɛ ir ɩ vʋr a ber ata daar.
42024047	Ban den a wʋ yuor mʋɔl kʋ nɩbʋrɔ ba jaa, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa lɩɛb a wʋ tɩɛr, Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ naa a wʋ yeldɛɛr bar, Jerusalɛm lɛ an piel.
42024048	Yɩn lɛ ɩ a anyãna dãasɩɛ dẽme.
42024049	A maa na tɩ tʋ̃ naa a 'lɔ a n Sãa na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ yɩ, tɩchɛ yɩ chɛnɛ jɩ̃nɛ a Jerusalɛm, ka a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ wa yi a saaju wa pɔɔ yɩ."
42024050	Wʋ tara ban yin tɩ gbʋrɔ nɩ a Betanɩ na wʋ tur a nuur saaju sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ ba.
42024051	A lɛ wʋn sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ba, wʋ bar ba naa ka Nãaŋmɩn 'mɔɔ wʋ don be a saaju.
42024052	A ba pãa gbʋr dumo puor wʋ tɩ lɩɛb pʋpɛl kul a Jerusalɛm.
42024053	Bɩbir jaa lɛ ba ma chen be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir tɩ dãna a Nãaŋmɩn.
43001001	A pielfʋ daar a 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a 'Yɛr ben be, ka a 'Yɛr be a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, ka a 'Yɛr ɩ Nãaŋmɩn.
43001002	Wʋ dɔ̃ɔ be a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ a pielfʋ daar.
43001003	A 'Yɛr nyã lɛ Nãaŋmɩn maal bomo a jaa. Bon jaa ba maal ka a ba tu a 'Yɛr nyã pɔ ɛ.
43001004	A wʋ pɔ lɛ nyɛvʋr be, a wʋ nyɛvʋr nyã lɛ kʋrɔ bomo a jaa chãa.
43001005	A chãa nyã lɛ chaara a libe pɔ, ka libe ba tʋ̃ɔ wʋ kpĩin ɛ.
43001006	Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃n daba na di Jɔɔn.
43001007	'Lɔ lɛ wa di a dãasɩɛ na wʋ 'yɛr a chãa nyã 'yɛr, ka a nɩrɛ jaa na tu a wʋ sɛ̃ sɔɔ de a chãa.
43001008	Jɔɔn ba ɩ a chãa ɛ, tɩ wʋ wa naa ɩka wʋ wa 'yɛr a chãa 'yɛr.
43001009	A yelmɩ̃ɛ chãa nyã lɛ chaara 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩrɛ jaa na waara a wɛr pɔ.
43001010	A 'yɛr dɔ̃ɔ be a wɛr pɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn gba maal a wɛr tu a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, tɩchɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ.
43001011	Wʋ wa naa a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ paal pɔ, tɩchɛ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ ba de wʋ ɛ.
43001012	Tɩchɛ nɩbɛ bamɩne de wʋ naa, na ba sɔɔ de a wʋ yuor, ka wʋ kʋ ba sɔr ka ba ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bibiir.
43001013	Baa ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bibiir nɩrɛ dɔɔfʋ kaar ɛ, bɩɩ nɩrɛ bɔfʋ pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ maal ba a wʋ bibiir.
43001014	A 'yɛr wa ɩ naa nɩrɛ na wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a sɩ sɛ̃. Sɩ nyɛ naa a wʋ tɩɩr, a tɩɩr nyã na ɩ a Sãa Bidabʋ̃'yen tɛɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ yi a Sãa sɛ̃ wa, na wʋ tara wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43001015	Jɔɔn 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr, na wʋ tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Nyã lɛ n 'yɛr yɩ ɩka wʋn wa naa, 'lɔ na be a n puor waara gar ma naa, bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ be be tɩ ba wa dɔɔ ma."
43001016	A wɩ̃ɛfʋ sɛɛ wʋ naa, ka a wʋ maal vɩla lʋɔr sɩ jaa bʋ̃'yen 'yen dɔɔlɔ taa waara a sɩ sɛ̃.
43001017	Bojũu, Mosesɩ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ waan a nɛɛ, tɩchɛ Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ lɛ waan a wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43001018	Nɩbʋ̃'yen jaa ba nyɛ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, tɩchɛ a Bidabʋ̃'yen tɛɛ 'lɔ na be a Sãa lõboor lɛ wiil sɩ a lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na be.
43001019	A nɩbɛrɛ na be a Jerusalɛm tʋ̃n a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlorbo nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ puorfʋ jie sʋ̃sʋ̃nbɔ ka ba tɩ sʋʋr Jɔɔn, nɩbuor lɛ wʋ ɩ,
43001020	Ka a Jɔɔn 'yɛr ba, "N ba ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃ ɩka wʋ wa faa a wʋ nɩbɛ ɛ."
43001021	Ka ba lɛ sʋʋr wʋ ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Elaija bɩɩ? Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "N ba ɩ wʋ ɛ." Ka ba lɛ sʋʋr wʋ ka 'lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɔ? Ka wʋ ɩka, "Kai."
43001022	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Tɩ an lɛ fʋ pãa ɩ? A sɩn tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a bala na tʋ̃ sɩ, 'yɛr sɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ fʋn ɩ."
43001023	Jɔɔn den a lɛ a Isaiya na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb na wʋ 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ a kɔkɔr 'lɔ na tãna a dãlpʋɔ pɔ, ɩka yɩ chɔɔr a Soro sɔr."
43001024	A Faraseemɩne tʋ̃n nɩbɛ bamɩne a Jɔɔn sɛ̃.
43001025	Ba wa sʋʋr wʋ naa, "Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ baa ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Nɩ-iraa ɛ, bɩɩ a Elaija ɛ, bɩɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ a fʋ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ?"
43001026	Be lɛ a Jɔɔn 'yɛr ba, "Maa den kʋ̃ɔ suoro nɩ a nɩbɛ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ ben a yɩ pɔ, yɩn ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
43001027	An ɩ maa lɛ de nie wa gba, n ba sɛɛ ɩka n for a wʋ nafɔbɔ mibe gba ɛ."
43001028	Jɔɔn be naa a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ puorfʋ jie suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, a Jordan man gɔ̃ɔn na be a Betanɩ, be lɛ wʋ 'yɛr a 'yɛr anyãna.
43001029	Wɛr na wa chaar, Jɔɔn nyɛn a Yesu na tor wʋ waara ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Pɛraabile, 'lɔ lɛ na de a wɛr nɩbɛ yeldɛbɛ bar.
43001030	Wʋ ɩ naa a 'lɔ ɩn 'yɛr ɩka, 'nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na wa naa, wʋ gar ma naa, bojũu 'lɔ dɔ̃ɔ be be tɩ ba wa dɔɔ ma.'
43001031	Maa ba bɔ̃ɔ a nɩnyɩnɛ wʋn ɩ ɛ, tɩ naa wa suoro yɩ nɩ kʋ̃ɔ ka bala jaa na be a Isɩral na nyɛ wʋ."
43001032	A Jɔɔn dãasɩɛ nɩ nyã, "N ben be nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na yi saaju fɩka ŋmam, wa 'mar wʋ, ka a Sɩɛ be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43001033	N ba dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a nɩnyɩnɛ wʋn ɩ ɛ. A 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma ɩka n wa suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ ma, 'A nɩrɛ 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋn wa nyɛ a Sɩɛ na suu wa 'mar na waa yi ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ na suoro a nɩbɛ nɩ a Sɩɛ.'
43001034	N nyɛn a anyã na ɩ, 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka 'lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bidabʋ̃'yen."
43001035	A wɛr na chaar go, Jɔɔn ara na a be nɩ a wʋ poturbo ayi.
43001036	Be lɛ wʋ nyɛ Yesu na tala, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Pɛraabile."
43001037	A Jɔɔn poturbo ayi bala na wõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr, ka ba turo a Yesu chiine.
43001038	Yesu na wa lɩɛb nyɛ ba, wʋ sʋʋr ba naa, "Bo yɩ bʋɔrɔ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Wiwile nyɩnɛ fʋ kpɩɛrɛ?"
43001039	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩ wa bɔ̃ɔ a jie." Ba jɩ̃nɛ naa a wʋ sɛ̃, bojũu mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ bal baar a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
43001040	A nɩbɛ ayi bala na wõ a lɛ Jɔɔn na 'yɛr ka ba turo a Yesu, ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ Andiru na ɩ a Simon Pita yɛbɛ.
43001041	Lɛ a Andiru na de nie ɩ lɛ, wʋ bɔ naa a wʋ yɛbɛ Simon 'yɛr wʋ, "Sɩ nyɛn a Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ na wa faa a wʋ nɩbɛ ban bʋɔlɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto."
43001042	Andiru tara naa a yɛbɛ waan a Yesu sɛ̃. Yesu na wa nyɛ wʋ, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Jɔɔn bidaba Simon, ban bʋɔlɔ fʋ naa Sɩfasɩ." A wʋ par lɛ Pita.
43001043	A ber anaar daar, Yesu chiine naa a Galilee, be lɛ wʋ nyɛ Filip na wʋ bʋɔl wʋ ɩka wʋ wa turo wʋ.
43001044	A Filip yin Betɩsaida, Andiru nɩ Pita tẽe.
43001045	Filip mɩ chen tɩ nyɛ Natanɩɛl 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Sɩ nyɛn a 'lɔ a Mosesɩ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na sɛb a wʋ yele, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ, Josefʋ bidaba."
43001046	Be lɛ a Natanɩɛl sʋʋr wʋ, "Yelsʋ̃ na tʋ̃ɔ yi a Najaretɩ tẽe ɔ?" Ka a Filip 'yɛr, "Wa kaa."
43001047	Yesu na wa nyɛ a Natanɩɛl na tor wʋ waara, wʋ 'yɛr naa, "Yɩ nyɛ a sɩ sãakpã Isɩral yɔ̃ɔ na ba tara bɛlfʋ ɛ."
43001048	Ka a Natanɩɛl sʋʋr a Yesu, "Ŋmɩnɛ fʋ ɩrɛ wa bɔ̃ɔ ma?" Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Filip na wa bʋɔlɔ fʋ, ka n nyɛ fʋ naa a kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ tɩɛ pĩlem."
43001049	Be lɛ a Natanɩɛl 'yɛr, "Wiwile, fʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn Bie nɩ a Isɩral Nãa."
43001050	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr sɔɔ wʋ, "Fʋ sɔɔ ma naa, bojũu ɩn 'yɛr ɩka n nyɛ fʋ naa a kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ tɩɛ pĩlem ɔ? Fʋn nyɛn yelbɛrɛ ka a gar lɛ.
43001051	Na wʋ 'yɛr, sɩrɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ ɩka fʋn nyɛn saaju na yuo ka a Nãaŋmɩn malakasɩ suro tɩ duoro a maa Nɩsaal Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ."
43002001	A ber a nyã puor, Yesu ma Mɛɛr be naa a pɔɔ ban kulo a tẽe na be a Galilee paal pɔ, ka ba bʋɔlɔ Keena.
43002002	Ba bʋɔl Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo ka ba mɩ be be a pɔɔ kulfʋ jie.
43002003	A dãa na wa baar, Mɛɛr 'yɛr kʋ Yesu, "A nɩbɛ dãa baar naa."
43002004	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "N ma, n sɔ̃ɔ ba ta ɛ, ta wiil ma a lɛ ɩn na ɩ ɛ."
43002005	Mɛɛr lɩɛb 'yɛr kʋ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ, "Yɩ ɩ lɛ Jaa a Yesu na wa 'yɛr ɩka yɩ ɩ."
43002006	Kʋsɩɛ dʋʋr ayʋɔb ben be, be lɛ a nɩbɛ ma ɔ̃ɔ a kʋ̃ɔ pɛɛ a ba mɩ̃ɛ lɛ a ba puorfʋ na ɩka ba ɩ. Yoi anaar bɩɩ anũu lɛ ma sɛɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa.
43002007	Yesu 'yɛr a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ɩka ba ɔ̃ɔ kʋ̃ɔ sɛɛ a dʋʋr.
43002008	An wa sɛɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ pãa ɔ̃ɔ a kʋ̃ɔ amɩne kʋ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ na kaara a pɔɔ paalaa yele." Ka a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ɩ a lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr ba.
43002009	Ka a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ na wa nyũ a kʋ̃ɔ ala na lɩɛb ɩ dãa, waa bɔ̃ɔ a jie a dãa na yi ɛ. A tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ 'lɔ bɔ̃ɔ naa. Be lɛ wʋ bʋɔl a pɔɔ paalaa sɩrɛ yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ,
43002010	na wʋ 'yɛr, "Nɩbɛ ma den nie waan a dãnʋ̃ɔ, bala wa nyũ tɩɩ baar, ka ba pãa waan a ala na ba bɔ̃ɔ nʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ. Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ bin a dãnʋ̃ɔ bar wa ta a baaraa."
43002011	A nɛ'maa yele nyã lɛ de nie Yesu na ɩ a Keena na be a Galilee paal pɔ. Be lɛ Yesu wiil a wʋ tɩɩr, ka a wʋ poturbo sɔɔ de wʋ.
43002012	A nyã puor, 'lɔ naa ma nɩ a wʋ yɛbil naa poturbo 'mantaa chen Kapenahum ɩka ba tɩ jɛ̃ bɩ̃lãa.
43002013	A kʋ̃ lɛ kor ɛ, ka a Juu nɩbɛ Gõl Bar Difʋ ta, Yesu don a Jerusalɛm.
43002014	Be lɛ wʋ tɩ nyɛ nɩbɛ na daara niin, piir nɩ papar, a Juu nɩbɛ puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ. Wʋ nyɛn bamɩne mɩ na jɛ̃n tɛɛbʋlsɩ tɛɛrɛ libie.
43002015	Wʋ den miir maal kpaara diin ba bar a puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, nɩ a ba piir nɩ a niin. Wʋ tɩɛ naa a libitɛɛrbɛ tɛɛbʋlsɩ lɔb ka a libie yɛ̃yɛl.
43002016	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a bala na daara a papar, "Yɩ yin a papar a ka, na yɩ ta maal ma a Sãa yir daa difʋ jie ɛ."
43002017	Ka a poturbo pãa tɩɛr tɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr, "Lɛ ɩn nʋ̃ a fʋ yir 'moro man fɩka bũu."
43002018	A Juu nɩbɛrɛ pãa sʋʋr a Yesu, "Jɩ̃nɛ buor lɛ fʋn maal wiil sɩ ka a ɩ fʋ tara na sɔr fʋn maal a lɛ?"
43002019	Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩ ŋmɛr a puorfʋ yir nyãna, tɩ ka n de ber ata mɛn wʋ go."
43002020	Ka a nɩbɛrɛ 'yɛr, "Yuom lɩjaayi nɩ ayʋɔb lɛ ba de mɛn a puorfʋ yir nyã, ŋmɩnɛ fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ de ber ata tɛɛ mɛn wʋ?"
43002021	Tɩchɛ a puorfʋ yir nyã a Yesu na 'yɛrɛ, ɩ naa a wʋ ɩ̃gãn lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ.
43002022	Yesu na wa ir a kũu pɔ, ka a wʋ poturbo tɩɛr yuo a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr, na ba pãa sɔɔ de lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr nɩ lɛ mɩ a Yesu na 'yɛr.
43002023	A be a Jerusalɛm a Gõl Bar Difʋ na wa ta, nɩyɔɔ sɔɔn de a wʋ yuor, bojũu ba nyɛn a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ wʋn tʋ̃.
43002024	Tɩchɛ Yesu na bɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ jaa tɩɛr, waa sɔɔ de wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ ba ɛ.
43002025	A ba ɩ nɩrɛ lɛ na 'yɛr wʋ lɛ nɩbɛ na be ɛ, bojũu wʋ bɔ̃ɔn nɩrɛ jaa tɩɛr.
43003001	Daba dɔ̃ɔ be be a Faraseemɩne pɔ, ka a wʋ yuor di Nikodimasɩ, wʋ mɩ ɩ naa a Juu nɩbɛ nɩdiere ɩ̃sʋɔ.
43003002	Wʋ dɔ̃ɔ chen a Yesu sɛ̃ tɩ̃sɔɔ na wʋ tɩ 'yɛr, "Wiwile, sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ tʋ̃ fʋ ɩka, fʋ wa wiil sɩ. Fʋ kʋ̃ naa tʋ̃ɔ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ anyãna tʋ̃ ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn ba be a fʋ sɛ̃ ɛ."
43003003	Ka a Yesu haa 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, fʋ̃ʋ ba nyɛ dɔɔ paalaa ɛ, fʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ."
43003004	A Nikodimasɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ban lɛ ɩ dɔɔ nɩkoraa gbɛɛ ayi? Wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a wʋ ma pʋɔ pɔ ka wʋ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ dɔɔ wʋ go ɛ."
43003005	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, fʋ̃ʋ na kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ, ka baa dɔɔ wʋ nɩ a kʋ̃ɔ nɩ a Sɩɛ ɛ.
43003006	A 'lɔ a nɩrɛ na dɔɔ ɩ naa nɩrɛ bie, Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ mɩ lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ nɩrɛ lɩɛb ka wʋ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bie.
43003007	Ta ɩ a nɛɛ 'maa fʋ ɩn 'yɛr ɩka a sɛɛ naa ka ba dɔɔfʋ dɔɔ paalaa ɛ.
43003008	Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ tɛɛ lɛ tɩrɛ a nyɛvʋr paalaa. A Sɩɛ kaar naa sɛsɛbɛ na furo chiine jie 'lɔ wʋn bʋɔrɔ, fʋn tʋ̃ɔn wõ a dɔɔn, tɩchɛ fʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a jie wʋn yi ɛ, bɩɩ a jie wʋn chiine ɛ."
43003009	Ka a Nikodimasɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Ŋmɩnɛ an ɩ wa ɩ a lɛ?"
43003010	Ka a Yesu haa 'yɛr, "Ŋmɩnɛ fʋ ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ wiwile tɩ ba bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna ɛ?
43003011	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, sɩ 'yɛrɛ naa ala sɩn bɔ̃ɔ, na sɩ di a ala sɩn 'yɛrɛ dãasɩɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba de a lɛ sɩn 'yɛr ɛ.
43003012	Ala ɩ yaa sɔɔ de a wɛr nyã bonsɩ 'yɛr ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ yɩn ɩrɛ wa sɔɔ de ala ɩ, n 'yɛr naa saaju bonsɩ 'yɛr?
43003013	Nɩrɛ ba do saaju jaa ɛ, ka a Nɩsaal Bie na yi a be wa tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
43003014	A Nɩsaal Bie na 'mɔɔn saaju nɩtãa lɛ a Mosesɩ na maal a kur jɩɛ 'mɔɔ a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ.
43003015	Ka nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na pãa sɔɔ de a Nɩsaal Bie na tara na nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
43003016	"Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃ naa a nɩbɛ na be ka a wɛr pɔ yɔɔ jaa, na wʋ de a wʋ Bidabʋ̃'yen tɛɛ kʋ sɩ, nɩrɛ jaa wa sɔɔ de wʋ, wʋ kʋ̃ wɛ ɛ, tɩ tara a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
43003017	Bojũu, Nãaŋmɩn ba tʋ̃ a wʋ Bidabʋ̃'yen nyã a wɛr pɔ ɩka wʋ wa sɔ̃ɔ a nɩbɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ wa naa ɩka wʋ wa faa ba.
43003018	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na wa sɔɔ de a Nãaŋmɩn Bidabʋ̃'yen nyã, wʋ kʋ̃ sɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ba wa sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ, wʋn sɔ̃ɔ wʋn bar, bojũu waa sɔɔ de a Nãaŋmɩn Bidabʋ̃'yen tɛɛ nyã yuor ɛ.
43003019	A baaraa nɩ nyã, chãa wan ka a wɛr pɔ, tɩchɛ a nɩbɛ nʋ̃n libe gar a chãa, bojũu a ba maalfʋ ɩn bier.
43003020	A nɩbɛ bala na ɩrɛ a bier 'laar chãa, ba kʋ̃ sɔɔ yi chãa pɔ ɛ, bojũu a chãa na wiil naa a lɛ ban be.
43003021	Tɩchɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na be be nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ma wan chãa pɔ, bojũu ba bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka a ba taaba ba bɔ̃ɔ ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ maala a lɛ ban maala."
43003022	A nyã puor, Yesu nɩ a wʋ poturbo 'mantaa chen Judiya be lɛ wʋ jɛ̃n ba bɩ̃lãa, na wʋ suoro nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
43003023	Jɔɔn mɩ dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ be a Ainon, a be ba jãa naa Salim ɛ, bojũu kʋ̃ɔ dɔ̃ɔ be be yɔɔ. Nɩbɛ dɔ̃ɔ chiine a wʋ sɛ̃ ka wʋ suoro ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
43003024	Baa na nyɔɔ a Jɔɔn pɔɔ sɛrɛ ɛ.
43003025	Jɔɔn poturbo bamɩne nɩ a Juu nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ chɩrɛ nɩ taa nɩ a ɩ̃gãn pɛɛfʋ yele.
43003026	Ba chen a Jɔɔn sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "Wiwile, fʋ 'yɛr a daba 'lɔ sɛ̃ fʋn dɔ̃ɔ be a Jordan man gɔ̃ɔn. Wʋ suoro na nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ka nɩrɛ jaa chiine a wʋ sɛ̃."
43003027	Ka Jɔɔn haa 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ bon jaa ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn na be a saaju baa sɔɔ ɛ.
43003028	Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ chɛnɛ na tɩɛr a ŋmɩnɛ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr yɩ ɩka n ba ɩ a Nɩ-iraa ɛ. Tɩchɛ wʋ tʋ̃ ma naa ka n de a wʋ nie.
43003029	A 'lɔ na kulo a pɔɔ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a pɔɔ sʋɔ. A wʋ bɩbɩɛlɛ pʋɔ ma pɛl naa wʋn ara a be wõnõ a pɔɔ sʋɔ kɔkɔr. Ala lɛ so ka a n pʋɔ mɩ pɛl.
43003030	A sɛɛ naa ɩka Yesu wʋ do, tɩchɛ ka maa suu.
43003031	"Nãaŋmɩn Bie nyã lɛ yi a saaju, 'lɔ lɛ gar ba jaa, nɩrɛ na yi ka a tẽe ɩn a tẽe tʋɔr na wʋ ma 'yɛrɛ a tẽe bomo 'yɛr. A 'lɔ na yi a saaju wa gar a bomo a jaa.
43003032	Wʋ ma 'yɛr naa a lɛ wʋn nyɛ nɩ a lɛ wʋn wõ tɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa maa sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ.
43003033	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na wa sɔɔ de, a wiil naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn ɩ naa yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ.
43003034	Bojũu, Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃ naa a wʋ Bie ka wʋ wa 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr. Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃ naa ka a wʋ Sɩɛ sɛɛ wʋ.
43003035	A Sãa nʋ̃ naa Bie na wʋ de yele a jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ nũu pɔ.
43003036	Nɩrɛ jaa na sɔɔ de a Bie tara na nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tɔr wʋ, ba tara a nyɛvʋr nyã ɛ, tɩ Nãaŋmɩn suur be a wʋ sɛ̃."
43004001	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a Faraseemɩne wõ naa wʋn nyɛrɛ nɩbɛ suoro ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ka a bala na turo wʋ gar a bala na turo a Jɔɔn.
43004002	Tɩchɛ Yesu poturbo lɛ dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, a ba ɩ Yesu mɩ̃ɛ lɛ ɛ.
43004003	Yesu bar naa Judiya tɩ lɩɛb chiine a Galilee go.
43004004	Ka a ɩ Samariya lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka wʋ tu.
43004005	A sɔr 'lɔ wʋn tu tɩ yi naa a Saika tẽe pɔ, na wʋ gbʋr a wɛr 'lɔ a Jekɔb na dɔ̃ɔ de kʋ a wʋ bidaba Josefʋ a kõr jaa.
43004006	A lɔ-ɔ̃ɔ a Jekɔb na dɔ̃ɔ tuu chɛnɛ na be be, ka a Yesu jɛ̃ gbʋr a lɔ-ɔ̃ɔ bojũu wʋ chen bal. Mɔ̃tɔ̃tuo sɔ̃ɔ lɛ.
43004007	Ka a Samariya pɔɔ suu a lɔ-ɔ̃ɔ pɔ kʋ̃ɔ ɔ̃ɔfʋ jie. Ka a Yesu sʋɔr wʋ, "Pɔɔ yãayãabɩlɛ, ɔ̃ɔ a kʋ̃ɔ kʋ ma ka n nyũ."
43004008	A Yesu poturbo mɩ kpɛ̃n a tẽe pɔ ɩka ba tɩ da bʋ̃diir.
43004009	Ka a Samariya pɔɔ 'yɛr, "Fʋ̃ʋ Juu nɩrɛ, maa mɩ Samariya pɔɔ, taa ɩ ŋmɩnɛ ka fʋ ɩka n kʋ fʋ kʋ̃ɔ ka fʋ nyũ," sɩn nɩ Juu nɩbɛ na ba mʋɔrɔ taa bũu ɛ?
43004010	A Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "Faa bɔ̃ɔ a bon a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ kʋ fʋ ɛ. Faa mɩ bɔ̃ɔ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sʋɔrɔ fʋ a kʋ̃ɔ ɩka wʋ nyũ ɛ, fʋ̃ʋ ta bɔ̃ɔ, fʋn taa sʋɔr man a kʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ na kʋrɔ nyɛvʋr."
43004011	A pɔɔ 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, faa tara bʋ̃-ɔ̃ɔnaa ɛ, ka a lɔ-ɔ̃ɔ mɩ yulʋ̃, nyɩnɛ lɛ fʋn nyɛ a kʋ̃ɔ ala na kʋrɔ a nyɛvʋr?
43004012	A sɩ sãakpã Jekɔb lɛ tuu a lɔ-ɔ̃ɔ nyãna kʋ sɩ, ka wʋ yɔn nɩ a wʋ dʋ̃n nyuro. Fʋ̃ʋ bɛrma gar a Jekɔb bɩɩ?"
43004013	Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na nyũ a kʋ̃ɔ nyãna, kɔ̃nyũur na kpɛ wʋ̃n go.
43004014	Tɩchɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na nyũ a kʋ̃ɔ ala ɩn na kʋ wʋ, kɔ̃nyũur kʋ̃ lɛ kpɛ wʋ go ɛ. A kʋ̃ɔ ala ɩn na kʋ wʋ kaara kɔ̃bulaa na yire, naa kʋrɔ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ."
43004015	Ka a pɔɔ 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ yãayãabɩlɛ, kʋ ma a kʋ̃ɔ ala ka n nyũ, ka a kɔ̃nyũur ta lɛ nyɔɔ ma ka n suu a lɔ-ɔ̃ɔ nyã pɔ go ɛ."
43004016	A Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "Kul tɩ tara a fʋ sɩrɛ waan."
43004017	Ka a pɔɔ 'yɛr, "N ma tara sɩrɛ ɛ." A Yesu 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ fʋ 'yɛr ɩka faa tara sɩrɛ ɛ.
43004018	Fʋ dɔ̃ɔ kul sɩrbɛ anũu, tɩ a daba 'lɔ sɛ̃ fʋn be a pʋ̃pãanyã ba ɩ a fʋ sɩrɛ ɛ."
43004019	Ka a pɔɔ 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ n nyɛ naa a fʋ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ.
43004020	A sɩ sãakpãmɩne, a tɔ̃ɔ nyã ju lɛ ba ma do tɩ puor a Nãaŋmɩn tɩchɛ a yɩn Juu nɩbɛ 'yɛr ɩka Jerusalɛm tɛɛ lɛ ɩ a puorfʋ jie."
43004021	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Pɔɔ sɔɔ de ma, sɔ̃ɔ waara an kʋ̃ ɩ a tɔ̃ɔ nyã ju bɩɩ Jerusalɛm yɩn do tɩ puor a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn go ɛ.
43004022	A yɩn Samariya nɩbɛ ba bɔ̃ɔ a 'lɔ yɩn puoro ɛ, a sɩn Juu nɩbɛ bɔ̃ɔ naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ sɩn puoro. Bojũu a sɩ jie lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na tu faa nɩbɛ.
43004023	Tɩchɛ a sɔ̃ɔ waara, wʋ gɔr ta baar, a bala na puoro a Nãaŋmɩn sɩrɛ jaa, a sɩɛ na wiil ba naa ka ba puor a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ. Ba nyãna puorfʋ lɛ a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔrɔ.
43004024	Nãaŋmɩn ɩn sɩɛ, bala na puoro wʋ a sɩɛ pɔ wʋn wiil ba naa ka ba puor wʋ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ pɔ."
43004025	Ka a pɔɔ 'yɛr, "N bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka a Nɩ-iraa na wa naa, a 'lɔ sɩn na bʋɔlɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto. 'Lɔ wa wa, wʋn wiil sɩ naa yele a jaa par."
43004026	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a pɔɔ, "Maa lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ nɩ fʋ̃ʋ na 'yɛrɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã."
43004027	Ka a ɩ a poturbo mɩ tɔ̃ɔ ta nyɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ nɩ a pɔɔ ka a nɛɛr 'maa ba. Tɩchɛ ba ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba 'la sʋʋr wʋ bo lɛ wʋ bʋɔrɔ bɩɩ bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ nɩ a pɔɔ ɛ.
43004028	A jie lɛ a pɔɔ bar a yuor tɩ jo kul a tẽe pɔ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ,
43004029	"Yɩ wa nyɛ daba na 'yɛr ma ala a jaa n na dɔ̃ɔ maal. Kaa 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa naa 'lɔ bɩɩ?"
43004030	Nɩrɛ jaa na be a tẽe pɔ yin chen na tɩ kaa a Yesu.
43004031	An wa ɩrɛ a lɛ ka a poturbo sʋɔr a Yesu. "Wiwile yãayãabɩlɛ, di bʋ̃diir."
43004032	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N tara na bʋ̃diir yɩn ba bɔ̃ɔ a yele ɛ."
43004033	Ka wʋ poturbo piel sʋrɔ taa, "Nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ tɔ̃ɔ waan bon kɔ̃ɔ wa kʋ wʋ ka wʋ di bɩɩ?"
43004034	A Yesu 'yɛr, "N bʋ̃diir lɛ ka n ɩ a lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ, 'lɔ lɛ tʋ̃ ma, ka n baar a tʋ̃mɔ̃ 'lɔ wʋn kʋ ma ɩka n tʋ̃.
43004035	Yɩn 'lɔ 'yɛr naa ɩka a chɛn ŋmɛrsɩ anaar ka a ŋmab ta, maa 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka, yɩ kaa yɩn nyɛn a por bonsɩ na mʋ̃ɔ sɛɛ ŋmab.
43004036	Pʋ̃pãanyã gba, a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ bala na ŋmara nyɛrɛ naa a ba sãyar, ban lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bʋ̃ŋmarsɩ waara nɩ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃. Ka a bala na bʋr a bʋ̃bie nɩ a ŋmaŋmarba pãa 'mataa chɩlɛ.
43004037	A sʋkpa na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka, bamɩne lɛ bʋr ka bamɩne mɩ ŋma.
43004038	Maa tʋ̃nɔ̃ yɩ naa ɩka, yɩ chen tɩ ŋma a puo 'lɔ pɔ a bamɩne na tʋ̃ hãn."
43004039	Nɩyɔɔ na yi a Samariya tẽe pɔ sɔɔn de Yesu, bojũu a pɔɔ 'yɛr kʋ ba ɩka, "A daba nyã 'yɛr naa a lɛ jaa n na dɔ̃ɔ maal."
43004040	Ba wan wa sʋɔr wʋ ɩka wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a ba tẽe, ka wʋ jɛ̃ be ber ayi.
43004041	A Samariya tẽe dẽme yɔɔ jie mɩ lɛ sɔɔn de Yesu bojũu ba wʋn a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr.
43004042	Be a ba 'yɛr kʋ a pɔɔ, "A ba ɩ lɛ fʋn 'yɛr kʋ sɩ jũu sɩ sɔɔ de a Yesu ɛ, sɩn mɩ̃ɛ wõ naa a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr kʋ sɩ, ka sɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka 'lɔ lɛ na faa a wɛr nɩbɛ."
43004043	A ber ayi na po, wʋ yin a be na wʋ chen Galilee.
43004044	Yesu 'yɛr naa, "Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ nyɛrɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ jie jaa, tɩchɛ a ba tẽe dẽme ba 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba ɛ."
43004045	Wʋn wa ta a Galilee, a nɩbɛ de wʋn nuur ayi a be, bojũu ba mɩ dɔ̃ɔ chen a Jerusalɛm a Gõl Bar Difʋ jie tɩ nyɛ a lɛ jaa wʋn maal.
43004046	Yesu na wa be a Galilee, wʋ lɩɛb chen a Keena tẽe pɔ be wʋn dɔ̃ɔ lɩɛb a kʋ̃ɔ ka a ɩ a dãa. Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kɔ̃ɔ ben Kapenahum ka a wʋ bie bɩɛrɛ.
43004047	Wʋn wa wõ ɩka a Yesu yin a Galilee wa a Judiya, wʋ chen tɩ sʋɔr wʋ ɩka wʋ sãa a wʋ bie na kpire.
43004048	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, "Yɩn baa nyɛ jɩ̃nɛ nɩ nɛ'maa yele ɛ, yɩ kʋ̃ sɔɔ de ɛ."
43004049	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, yãayãabɩlɛ, wa ka a n bie ta kpi ɛ."
43004050	A Yesu pãa 'yɛr, "A fʋ bie sa naa, kulo a yir." A daba sɔɔn de a lɛ a Yesu na 'yɛr na wʋ lɩɛb kulo a yir.
43004051	Ka a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ na yi a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ yir tuor wʋ a sɔr pɔ 'yɛr, "A fʋ bie sa naa."
43004052	A wʋ sʋʋr ba a sɔ̃ɔ buor a bie na sa, ka ba 'yɛr, "Jãa mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na vɩrʋ̃ lɛ a ɩ̃gãn tul bar wʋ."
43004053	Ka a bie sãa tɩɛr tɔ an ɩ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ vɩr naa a jãa, a Yesu na 'yɛr, "A fʋ bie sa naa." A daba naa bala ba jaa na be a wʋ yir sɔɔn de a Yesu.
43004054	A nɛ'maa yelsɩ ayi lɛ anyã Yesu na tʋ̃ wʋn yi a Judiya na wʋ chen a Galilee.
43005001	A anyã puor, a Juu nɩbɛ tara na lɔ̃ɔ di ka a Yesu chen a be a Jerusalɛm.
43005002	A tẽe pɔ, gbatarbile ben be ka a jɛ̃bɛrsɩ anũu be be. A jie gbʋr a be ban bʋɔlɔ a piir dɔ̃dɔr, ka a Juu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr pɔ a ba bʋɔlɔ Betesda.
43005003	A jɛ̃bɛrsɩ ala pɔ baal bʋrsɩ ben be, jɔ̃n, bamɩne gbɛɛ na kpi kpi nɩ gbɛrsɩ ka ba gã kɔɔ a kʋ̃ɔ.
43005005	A gbatarbile 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ koor mɩ lɛ nɩbaala na bɛ yuom lɩjɛr nɩ pie nɩ aniin (38) na wʋ gã a be.
43005006	Yesu na wa nyɛ a daba, wʋ bɔ̃ɔn naa wʋn gbɛr kor, ka wʋ sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka fʋ sa bɩɩ?"
43005007	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, n ba tara nɩrɛ na 'mɔɔ ma 'yɔ̃ɔ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ 'lɔ wa dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ, n ma mʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n kpɛ, tɩchɛ ka a nɩrɛ ma dɔ̃ɔ ma nie kpɛ."
43005008	A Yesu pãa 'yɛr wʋ, "'Mɔɔ a fʋ bʋ̃gãnaa chiine."
43005009	Ajienaa ka a daba sa, na wʋ 'mɔɔ a sɔ̃ɔ chiine. A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir daar lɛ a anyãna ɩ.
43005010	A Juu nɩbɛrɛ na wa nyɛ a daba na tuo a sɔ̃ɔ, ka ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir lɛ, nɩrɛ jaa ba tara sɔr ɩka wʋ tuo a wʋ sɔ̃ɔ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir ɛ."
43005011	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr, "A daba 'lɔ na sa ma lɛ 'yɛr kʋ ma ɩka n 'mɔɔ a sɔ̃ɔ chiine."
43005012	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Nɩbuor lɛ 'yɛr fʋ ɩka fʋ 'mɔɔ a sɔ̃ɔ tuo chiine?"
43005013	A daba ba dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a Yesu a nɩbuor wʋn ɩ ɛ, Yesu kpɛ̃n a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ.
43005014	A nyã puor, a Yesu nyɛn a daba a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir pɔ na wʋ 'yɛr wʋ, "Fʋ pãa sãn pʋ̃pãanyã, taa wa ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr go ɛ, ka amɩne wa pɔɔ fʋ gar a lɛ ɛ."
43005015	Ka a daba chen tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Juu nɩbɛrɛ, Yesu lɛ ɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sa ma.
43005016	Ba piel bʋɔrɔ sɔɩ na ɩ Yesu yele bojũu wʋ ma tʋ̃nɔ̃ naa a anyãna a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar.
43005017	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr ba, "N Sãa ba vɛ̃ anyãna tʋ̃fʋ ɛ, ala lɛ so ka n mɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃."
43005018	A nɩbɛrɛ tara na yele ayi ban bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba kõn Yesu. Wʋ sɔ̃ɔ naa a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir yele, tɩchɛ a dɛɛr 'lɔ jaa lɛ wʋn 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn ɩ naa a wʋ Sãa, na wʋ de a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ka 'lɔ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn ɩ bʋ̃'yen.
43005019	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka a Bie kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ maal bon jaa ɛ. Wʋn tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a lɛ tɛɛ wʋn nyɛ a Sãa na maala, bojũu a Bie ma maal naa a lɛ nɛ wʋn nyɛ a Sãa na maala.
43005020	A Sãa nʋ̃n a Bie na wʋ wiil wʋ a yele a jaa wʋn maal. A Sãa gba na wiil wʋn yelbɛrɛ ka yɩ nɛɛr 'maa.
43005021	A lɛ a Sãa na ma sɩ̃ɩ a kũu na wʋ kʋ wʋ nyɛvʋr, lɛ lɛ a Bie mɩ na kʋ a ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋn bʋɔrɔ a nyɛvʋr.
43005022	A Sãa gba ba tɔɔrɔ nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ɩka a Bie wʋ tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr.
43005023	A Sãa bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Bie nɩtãa lɛ ban 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ. Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa tɔr ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a Bie ɛ, lɛ mɩ lɛ wʋ tɔr, ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a Sãa na tʋ̃ wʋ ɛ.
43005024	"Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na wõ a lɛ ɩn na 'yɛr tɩ sɔɔ de a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma, tara na nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃. Ba kʋ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ 'yɛr ɛ. Wʋ yin kũu pɔ, tɩ kpɛ nyɛvʋr pɔ.
43005025	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, sɔ̃ɔ waara, wʋ ben ta ka a kũn na wõ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie kɔkɔr. A bala na wõ naa, na ir tara nyɛvʋr.
43005026	Bojũu a Sãa tara na kpɛ̃ɔ kʋrɔ nyɛvʋr. Wʋ den a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ kʋ a Bie ka wʋ mɩ tara nyɛvʋr.
43005027	Wʋ kʋ wʋn sɔr ɩka wʋ tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr, bojũu wʋ ɩ naa Nɩsaal Bie.
43005028	"Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a 'maa yɩ nɛɛ ɛ. A sɔ̃ɔ na wa naa, ka a kũn wõ a Nɩsaal Bie kɔkɔr,
43005029	na ba yire a ba yar pɔ. Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na maal vɩla, na yin kpɛ nyɛvʋr pɔ, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mɩ na maal dɛɛr na yin kpɛ sɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ.
43005030	N kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ maal bon jaa nɩ maa mɩ̃ɛ kpɛ̃ɔ ɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ 'yɛr ma a lɛ ɩn na tɔɔrɔ ka a n tɔɔrfʋ tara sɔr bojũu n turo naa a wʋ nɛɛ, a ba ɩ n ɩrɛ na lɛ ɩn bʋɔrɔ ɛ.
43005031	"Maa 'yɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a n mɩ̃ɛ, sɔr jaa ba be be na wiil ɩka yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ ɛ.
43005032	Nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ ben be na 'yɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma, ka n mɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43005033	"Yɩ tʋ̃n nɩbɛ a Jɔɔn sɛ̃ ka wʋ tɩ 'yɛr ba a yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43005034	N ba dɩɛl lɛ nɩbɛ na 'yɛrɛ a n 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ yɩ naa anyãna ka yɩ na tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ faafʋ.
43005035	Jɔɔn dɔ̃ɔ ɩ fɩka fɩ̃tɩn na chaar yɔ̃ɔ ka yɩ pʋɔ pɛl, a yɩ chɩl a chãa nyã pɔ bɩ̃lãa.
43005036	"Bon kɔ̃ɔ na tɩrɛ gar a lɛ a Jɔɔn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a n 'yɛr, naa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala a Sãa na kʋ ma ɩka n tʋ̃. A anyãna a jaa 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ ma, naa wiil ɩka a Sãa lɛ tʋ̃ ma.
43005037	A Sãa mɩ na tʋ̃ ma 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ ma, tɩchɛ yaa wõ a wʋ kɔkɔr bɩɩ nyɛ a wʋ nie jaa ɛ.
43005038	Yaa sɔɔ a wʋ 'yɛr ɛ, bojũu yɩ tɔr na yaa sɔɔ de a 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃ ɛ.
43005039	Yɩ ma chɛ̃pɛ̃ naa a Nãaŋmɩn gãma, bojũu yɩ tɩɛr naa ɩka be lɛ yɩn nyɛ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. Maa 'yɛr lɛ a gãma anyãna 'yɛrɛ.
43005040	Tɩchɛ yɩ tɔr naa na wa a n sɛ̃ wa nyɛ nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
43005041	"N baka ba be nɩrɛ pɛɛfʋ pɔ ɛ.
43005042	Tɩchɛ n bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba nʋ̃ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ.
43005043	Maa waan naa a n Sãa yuor, ka yaa de ma ɛ. Tɩchɛ yɩn den nɩbɛ na waan ba mɩ̃ɛ yuor.
43005044	Ŋmɩnɛ yɩn ɩrɛ wa sɔɔ? Yɩn na bʋɔrɔ ɩka a yɩ barmɩne ba pɛɛrɛ yɩ, ka yɩ baka ba be a pɛɛfʋ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ na kʋ yɩ ɛ.
43005045	"Tɩchɛ, yɩ taa tɩɛr ɩka ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩn 'yɛr a Sãa niem ɛ. Yɩ den a yɩ tɩɛr dɔɔl Mosesɩ, 'lɔ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ 'yɛr.
43005046	Maa 'yɛr lɛ a Mosesɩ na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb, ala ɩ yɩn ta sɔɔ wʋ, yɩn taa sɔɔ ma naa.
43005047	Tɩchɛ yɩn ba sɔɔ a lɛ a Mosesɩ na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ yɩn ɩrɛ wa sɔɔ a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr?"
43006001	A anyã puor, Yesu gɔ̃ɔ naa a Galilee man gɔ̃ɔn be ban bʋɔlɔ a Tiberiyas.
43006002	Nɩyɔɔ tu wʋn chen ban nyɛ wʋn tʋ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ na wʋ sãa baalsɩ.
43006003	Ka a Yesu pãa do a tɔ̃ɔ ju, na wʋ tɩ jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a wʋ poturbo.
43006004	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ Gõl Bar Difʋ mɩ gbʋr.
43006005	Yesu na wa nyɛ a nɩyɔɔ ka ba waara a wʋ sɛ̃, wʋ sʋʋr Filip, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ sɩn nyɛ bʋ̃diir kʋ a nɩbɛ banyãna?"
43006006	Wʋ sʋʋr a nɩtɔ̃ ɩka wʋ bɛɛr a Filip kaa, tɩ bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ wʋn na ɩ.
43006007	Ka a Filip 'yɛr, "Faa bɔ̃ɔ ka an den ŋmɛrsɩ aniin sãyar a fʋn dãn paanʋ̃ɔ jaa pʋʋr kʋ a nɩbɛ banyãna ɛ?"
43006008	Andiru na ɩ a Simon Pita yɛbɛ, a Yesu poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ, ka wʋ 'yɛr.
43006009	"Dabile ben ka na wʋ tara a chi jɔ̃n paanʋ̃ɔ anũu nɩ jɩ̃mɛ ayi, tɩ bo an maal a nɩyɔɔ banyãna?"
43006010	Mʋɔr pɔɔn a tẽe wʋ jaa, ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo ka ba ɩ a nɩbɛ jɩ̃nɛ jɩ̃nɛ. A nɩbɛ bala dɔ̃ɔ ɩ tur anũu (5,000).
43006011	Yesu den a paanʋ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ nũu pɔ tɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, tɩ de a paanʋ̃ɔ põ a nɩbɛ, na wʋ lɛ de a jɩ̃mɛ mɩ põ ba.
43006012	Ka a nɩbɛ di lɛ ban bʋɔrɔ, ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo ɩka ba wob a bʋ̃ŋmaara ala na chɛ, ka a bon jaa ta wɛ ɛ.
43006013	Lɛ lɛ ba wob a ala na chɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ pɛr pie nɩ ayi a chi paanʋ̃ɔ anũu ala.
43006014	A nɩbɛ na wa nyɛ a anyã baar lɛ a Yesu na tʋ̃ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃, ba piel 'yɛrɛ, "A nyã lɛ tɔ̃ɔ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ 'lɔ na wa a wɛr pɔ."
43006015	Yesu na wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka ba bʋɔrɔ naa na fɩr wʋ ka wʋ ɩ a ba nãa, wʋ don a tɔ̃ɔ ju wʋ yõ.
43006016	A jãanʋɔr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, a Yesu poturbo lɩɛb suu a man pɔ.
43006017	Na ba tɩ kpɛ a gboro pɔ piel gɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Kapenahum. A jãanɔ'maar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ Yesu ba wa a ba sɛ̃ sɛrɛ ɛ.
43006018	A sɛsɛkpɛ̃ɛ furo na ka a kʋ̃ɔ dãdaala.
43006019	Ka a poturbo na wa mɔ̃ kpɛ sɔɔ jaa, ba nyɛn a Yesu na chiine a kʋ̃ɔ ju waara a gboro par ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba.
43006020	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Maa lɛ, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ."
43006021	Ka ba ta ɩka ba de wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a gboro pɔ, tɩ ajienaa ka a gboro mɩ ta a gogoro nɛɛ a jie 'lɔ ban chiine.
43006022	A wɛr na wa chaar, a nɩyɔɔ bala na jɩ̃nɛ a man gɔ̃ɔn bɔ̃ɔn na ɩka gboro bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be. Ka Yesu naa poturbo ba 'mataa kpɛ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ bala tɛɛ lɛ chiine.
43006023	Ka gboi amɩne na yi Tiberiyas wa ara gbʋr a be a Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan tɩ ka a nɩbɛ di a bʋ̃diir.
43006024	A nɩbɛ na wa nyɛ ka a Yesu bɩɩ a wʋ poturbo ba be be ɛ, ba kpɛ̃n a gboi ala chiine a Kapenahum na tɩ bɔ a Yesu.
43006025	Ban wa tɩ nyɛ wʋ a manyal gɔ̃ɔn, ba sʋʋr wʋ naa, "Wiwile, dabor fʋ wa ka?"
43006026	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋ̃rɔ yɩ, yɩ yʋɔrɔ na bʋɔrɔ ma a ba ɩ a nɛ 'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ yɩn nyɛ ɩn tʋ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bʋ̃diir yɩn di tɩɩ jũu.
43006027	Yɩ ta tʋ̃nɔ̃ bʋɔrɔ bʋ̃diir anyã na sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ bʋɔrɔ bʋ̃diir anyã na kʋ yɩ nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, ala lɛ a maa Nɩsaal Bie na kʋ yɩ. Bojũu 'lɔ lɛ a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn kʋ sɔr ɩka wʋ ɩ a lɛ."
43006028	Be lɛ ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Bãa lɛ sɩn na ɩ na sɩ tʋ̃ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ?"
43006029	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ nyã ɩka yɩ sɔɔ de a 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃."
43006030	Lɛ lɛ ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Nɛ'maa tʋ̃buor lɛ fʋn tʋ̃ ka sɩ nyɛ tɩ sɔɔ de fʋ? Bo lɛ fʋn ɩ?
43006031	A sɩ sãakpãmɩne din a maana a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb. Wʋ kʋ ba naa a bʋ̃diir na yi saaju ka ba di."
43006032	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a ba ɩ Mosesɩ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ kʋ yɩ a bʋ̃diir ala na yi a saaju ɛ, tɩchɛ a n Sãa lɛ dɔ̃ɔ kʋ yɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ bʋ̃diir ala na yi a saaju.
43006033	A Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃diir ɩ naa a 'lɔ na yi a saaju wa, na wʋ wa kʋrɔ a wɛr nɩbɛ nyɛvʋr."
43006034	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, an yi a dɩna tɩ chiine, kʋrɔ sɩ a bʋ̃diir ala."
43006035	Be a Yesu pãa 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ a bʋ̃diir ala na kʋrɔ nyɛvʋr, 'lɔ jaa na wa n sɛ̃ kʋ̃ lɛ chiin kɔ̃ ɛ. 'Lɔ jaa mɩ na sɔɔ de ma, kɔ̃nyũur kʋ̃ lɛ kpɛ wʋ ɛ.
43006036	Tɩchɛ a lɛ n na 'yɛr kʋ yɩ, yɩ nyɛ ma naa tɩ yaa sɔɔ de ma ɛ.
43006037	Bala ba jaa a Sãa na kʋ ma, ban wan a n sɛ̃. Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mɩ wa wa a n sɛ̃, n kʋ̃ dii wʋ bar ɛ.
43006038	Bojũu, n ba yi a saaju wa ɩka n wa ɩ a n bɔfʋ ɛ, tɩ n wa naa ɩka n wa ɩ a Sãa bɔfʋ. 'Lɔ lɛ tʋ̃ ma.
43006039	A nyã lɛ ɩ a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma bɔfʋ, ka n taa ɩrɛ wa vɛ̃ ka bala jaa wʋn kʋ ma bɔr ɛ, tɩchɛ ka n sɩ̃ɩ ba, ka ba ir ɩ vʋɛ a ber baaraa daar.
43006040	Bojũu, a n Sãa bɔfʋ nɩ nyã ɩka, nɩrɛ jaa na kaa a Bie na wʋ sɔɔ de wʋ, ban tara naa a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, ka n sɩ̃ɩ ba, ka ba ir ɩ vʋɛ a ber baaraa daar."
43006041	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ piel hũhũnõ bojũu a Yesu 'yɛr ɩka, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a bʋ̃diir 'lɔ na yi a saaju wa.
43006042	Ka ba 'yɛrɛ, "A ba ɩ a Yesu lɛ a nyã ɛ, a Josefʋ bidaba, a wʋ sãa nɩ a wʋ ma sɩn bɔ̃ɔ ɛ? Ŋmɩnɛ wʋ ɩrɛ wa 'yɛr ɩka saaju lɛ n yi wa?"
43006043	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr ba, "Yɩ bar a hũhũfʋ.
43006044	Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wa a n sɛ̃ ɛ, ka a Sãa na tʋ̃ ma baa tɔɔ wʋ waan ɛ, ka n sɩ̃ɩ wʋ ka wʋ ir ɩ vʋr a ber baaraa daar.
43006045	A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ dɔ̃ɔ sɛb, 'Nãaŋmɩn na wiil ba jaa.' Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na chɛlɛ a Sãa sɛ̃, na wʋ jãn yi a wʋ sɛ̃, na wa naa a n sɛ̃.
43006046	Nɩrɛ jaa ba nyɛ a Sãa ɛ, a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, 'lɔ tɛɛ lɛ nyɛ a Sãa.
43006047	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔɔ de ma tara na nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
43006048	Maa lɛ ɩ a bʋ̃diir ala na tara nyɛvʋr.
43006049	A yɩ sãakpãmɩne dɔ̃ɔ di a maana a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ tɩ chɛnɛ kpi.
43006050	Tɩchɛ a bʋ̃diir 'lɔ na yi a saaju wa nɩ nyã, 'lɔ lɛ nɩrɛ na di na wʋ kʋ̃ kpi ɛ.
43006051	Maa lɛ ɩ a nyɛvʋr bʋ̃diir 'lɔ na yi a saaju wa. Ala ɩ nɩrɛ di naa a bʋ̃diir nyãna, wʋn ben be jaa kpo kpo. A bʋ̃diir nyã ɩ naa a n ɩ̃gãn ɩn de kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ na be a wɛr pɔ, ka ba na nyɛ nyɛvʋr."
43006052	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ piel chɩrɛ taa nɩ suur na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a daba nyãna na ɩrɛ wa kʋ sɩ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn ka sɩ 'wɔb?"
43006053	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ. Yɩn baa 'wɔb a Nɩsaal Bie ɩ̃gãn na yɩ nyũ a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ ɛ, yaa tara nyɛvʋr ɛ.
43006054	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na 'wɔb a n ɩ̃gãn na wʋ nyũ a n jɩ̃ɩ tara na a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, tɩ ka n sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a wʋ ir ɩ vʋr a ber baaraa daar.
43006055	A n ɩ̃gãn ɩ naa bʋ̃dimɩ̃ɛ, ka n jɩ̃ɩ mɩ ɩ bʋ̃nyũmɩ̃ɛ.
43006056	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na 'wɔb a n ɩ̃gãn na wʋ nyũ a n jɩ̃ɩ, be naa a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ka n mɩ be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43006057	Nɩtãa lɛ a Sãa na ɩ a nyɛvʋr sʋɔ na tʋ̃ ma ka n be be a Sãa jũu, nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na 'wɔb ma mɩ na ben be a maa jũu.
43006058	A bʋ̃diir nyã lɛ yi a saaju wa. Sɩ sãakpãmɩne dɔ̃ɔ di a maana tɩ kpi, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na di a bʋ̃diir nyã na ben be kpo kpo."
43006059	Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ wile ba a Juu nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir a Kapenahum ala lɛ wʋ 'yɛr a nyãna.
43006060	Yesu poturbo yɔɔ na wa wõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr, ka ba 'yɛr, "A fʋ wiilfʋ nyã kpɛ̃mɛ na kpɛ, an lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ de?"
43006061	Yesu na bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ a poturbo na hũhũnõ, ka wʋ sʋʋr ba, "A nɩtɔ̃ chɛ yɩn bɩɩ?
43006062	Ŋmɩnɛ an pãa kaara, yɩn wa nyɛ a Nɩsaal Bie na duoro a jie 'lɔ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ be?
43006063	'Lɔ na kʋrɔ a nɩrɛ nyɛvʋr ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ. Nɩrɛ mɩ̃ɛ fɔ̃ɔ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ maal bon jaa ɛ. A 'yɛr ala ɩn 'yɛr yɩ, ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr, naa ɩ Nyɛvʋr.
43006064	Tɩchɛ a yɩ bamɩne ba sɔɔ ɛ." Bojũu, Yesu bɔ̃ɔn naa a pielfʋ a 'lɔ na ba sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ, nɩ a 'lɔ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ.
43006065	Be lɛ wʋ 'yɛr, "Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ so ka n 'yɛr ɩka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wa a n sɛ̃ ɛ, ka a Sãa baa waan wʋ ɛ."
43006066	An yi a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a poturbo yɔɔ ŋmaan yi na baa lɛ turo wʋ go ɛ.
43006067	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr a Pie Nɩ Ayi bala, "A yɩn mɩ, yɩ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yi ŋmaa yi bɩɩ?"
43006068	Be a Simon Pita 'yɛr, "N Soro, an sɛ̃ lɛ sɩn chen? An ɩ fʋ̃ʋ tɛɛ lɛ tara a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
43006069	Sɩ sɔɔn de na sɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka fʋ ɩ naa a chɛchɛ sʋɔ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃."
43006070	Ka a Yesu haa 'yɛr, "A ba ɩ maa lɛ ir a yɩ Pie Nɩ Ayi ɛ? Tɩchɛ ka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩ Satan tʋɔr."
43006071	Wʋ 'yɛrɛ naa a Judas na ɩ a Pie Nɩ Ayi ɩ̃sʋɔ na wa gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ. Wʋ ɩ naa a Simon bidaba na yi Isɩkariyot.
43007001	A anyã puor, Yesu yi naa Judiya tɩ yʋɔrɔ a Galilee paal pɔ, bojũu a Juu nɩbɛ bʋɔrɔ naa a wʋ kʋfʋ.
43007002	Tɩchɛ a Juu nɩbɛ sɛɛr pɔ lɔ̃ɔ di bɩbir na wa gbʋrɔ,
43007003	a Yesu yɛbil 'yɛr wʋ naa, "Yi a ka chen a Judiya ka a fʋ poturbo mɩ tɩ nyɛ a fʋ nɛ 'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃.
43007004	Nɩrɛ jaa na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bʋɔlɔ a wʋ yuor ba sɔɔlɔ ɛ. Fʋn maala a nyãna, wiil a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ka nɩbɛ jaa nyɛ fʋ."
43007005	Bojũu a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yɛbil ba sɔɔ de wʋ gba ɛ.
43007006	A lɛ jũu, a Yesu 'yɛr ba, "A n bɩbir ba vɩɛ ɛ, yɩn bɩbir vɩɛ naa.
43007007	A wɛr nɩbɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'laar yɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ ba 'laar ma naa bojũu n 'yɛr ba naa ɩka a lɛ ban ɩrɛ ɩn dɛɛr.
43007008	Yɩn, yɩ chiine a lɔ̃ɔ di jie. Maa ba chiine a lɔ̃ɔ di jie sɛrɛ ɛ, bojũu n bɩbir ba vɩɛ ɛ."
43007009	Wʋ 'yɛr naa lɛ tɩ chɛnɛ jɩ̃nɛ a Galilee.
43007010	A wʋ yɛbil na wa chen a lɔ̃ɔ di jie baar ka wʋ mɩ ir sɔɔl chen.
43007011	A lɔ̃ɔ di jie lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ jʋrɔ wʋ tɩ sʋrɔ taa, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ a daba 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ be?"
43007012	A nɩyɔɔ bala bʋlɔ na 'yɛrɛ kʋ̃rɔ taa, "A Yesu ɩn nɩsʋ̃." Ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Nɩbɛlɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ."
43007013	Tɩchɛ baa 'lara 'yɛrɛ ka a yire chãa pɔ ɛ, bojũu ba joro naa a Juu nɩbɛrɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ.
43007014	A lɔ̃ɔfʋ na wa põ jɩ̃taa, Yesu don kpɛ a Juu nɩbɛ puorfʋ jie na wʋ tɩ piel wile.
43007015	Ka a nɛɛr 'maa a Juu nɩbɛrɛ ka ba sʋrɔ taa, "Ŋmɩnɛ a daba nyã ɩrɛ wa bɔ̃ɔ a nɩtɔ̃ wʋn ba jãn ɛ?"
43007016	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A wiilfʋ nyã ba yi a n sɛ̃ ɛ, a yi naa a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma sɛ̃.
43007017	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kaa ir ɩka wʋn ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ, wʋn bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka a wiilfʋ nyã yin Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ bɩɩ n mɩ̃ɛ lɛ n wile.
43007018	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'yɛrɛ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr, bʋɔrɔ na 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋrɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ. Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tʋ̃nɔ̃ bʋɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋrɔ a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ wʋ, a nɩnyɩnɛ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ ka a bɛlfʋ ba be a wʋ jie ɛ.
43007019	Mosesɩ baa dɔ̃ɔ bin a Nɛɛ kʋ yɩ ɛ? Tɩ yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba tʋ̃ɔ tu ɛ. Bo 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ kʋ ma?"
43007020	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala 'yɛr, "Sɩdɛɛr lɛ fʋ tara, an bʋɔrɔ fʋ kʋfʋ?"
43007021	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Gbɛbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ n be tʋ̃, tɩchɛ ka a be 'maa yɩ a nɛɛ a nɩtɔ̃?
43007022	Mosesɩ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ wiil yɩ a yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ an ba ɩ 'lɔ sɛ̃ lɛ a dɔ̃ɔ yi ɛ, tɩ yi a sãakpãmɩne sɛ̃, ka ba ma ŋmaa yʋɔr a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar.
43007023	Ala ɩ yɩn tʋ̃ɔ ŋmaa bibile yʋɔr a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar tɩ ka a Mosesɩ nɛɛ 'lɔ wʋn bin ba sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, bo lɛ so ka yɩ nyɛ suur 'yɔ̃ɔ ma nɩrɛ ɩn sa a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar?
43007024	Yɩ ta bʋ̃nɔ̃ tɔɔr ɛ, tɩ yɩ tɔɔrɔ a lɛ na tor."
43007025	Nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi Jerusalɛm piel sʋrɔ taa, "A ba ɩ a daba nyã lɛ ba bʋɔrɔ a kʋfʋ ɛ,
43007026	nyɛ wʋn ara 'yɛrɛ chãa pɔ, ka baa 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr ɛ? A nɩbɛrɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka 'lɔ lɛ a Nɩ-iraa bɩɩ?
43007027	Tɩchɛ sɩn bɔ̃ɔ naa a jie 'lɔ a daba nyãna na yi. A Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ wa wa, nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔ a jie wʋn na yi ɛ."
43007028	Yesu chɛnɛ na wile a be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, na wʋ tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Ɔ̃ɔ yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ma naa, na yɩ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ a jie 'lɔ n na yi. N ba be ka nɩ n mɩ̃ɛ kpɛ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, yɩn ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
43007029	Tɩchɛ maa bɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa, wʋ sɛ̃ lɛ n yi, 'lɔ lɛ tʋ̃ ma."
43007030	A anyã lɛ ba ta bʋɔrɔ a wʋ nyɔɔfʋ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ jaa ba lɩɛb wʋ nũu sɩɩr wʋ ɛ, bojũu a wʋ bɩbir ba vɩɛ ɛ.
43007031	A nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ, bamɩne chɛnɛ na sɔɔ de wʋ na ba 'yɛrɛ, "A Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ wa wa, wʋn tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ gar a daba nyã bɩɩ?"
43007032	Faraseemɩne wõn a lɛ a nɩyɔɔ bala na bʋlɔ 'yɛrɛ a Yesu 'yɛr, ka a bala naa Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ tʋ̃ a puorfʋ yir kakaarba ka ba tɩ nyɔɔ wʋ waan.
43007033	Be a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N be naa yɩ sɛ̃ bɩ̃lãa, tɩ naa pãa lɛ lɩɛb chen a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma sɛ̃.
43007034	Yɩn wa yʋɔrɔ na bʋɔrɔ ma, tɩchɛ yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ ma ɛ, a be n na be yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wa be ɛ."
43007035	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ pãa sʋrɔ taa, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ a daba nyã na pãa chen ka sɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ wʋ ɛ? Wʋn chen naa be a sɩ nɩbɛ na yaar jɛr a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ tɩ wile ba bɩɩ?
43007036	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ wʋ 'yɛr ɩka, yɩn wa yʋɔrɔ na bʋɔrɔ ma tɩ yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ ma ɛ, a be n na be yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wa be ɛ."
43007037	A bɩbir baaraa daar na ɩ a lɔ̃ɔ di bɩbir kpɛ̃ɛ, Yesu ir ara tɩ tãn 'yɛr, "Kɔ̃nyũur wa kpɛ nɩrɛ, wʋ wa a n sɛ̃ wa nyũ.
43007038	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de ma nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr, nyɛvʋr kʋ̃ɔ na joro na yire a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ."
43007039	Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr lɛ wʋ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ, a bala na sɔɔ de wʋ ka wʋn kʋ ba. A Sɩɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ wa ɛ, an ɩ a Yesu ba nyɛ a tɩɩr sɛrɛ ɛ.
43007040	A nɩbɛ na wa wõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr, ka bamɩne 'yɛr, "A daba nyã ɩn Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ yelmɩ̃ɛ."
43007041	Ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛrɛ, "A nyã lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Nɩ-iraa." Ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ na ɩrɛ wa yi Galilee?
43007042	Nãaŋmɩn gãn ba 'yɛr ɩka David yɔ̃ɔ lɛ wʋn ɩ na wʋ yi Bɛtɩlɛhɛm, a tẽe 'lɔ a David na dɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ ɛ?"
43007043	Ka a nɩbɛ ŋma dẽ dẽ a Yesu juu.
43007044	Bamɩne mɩ ta bʋɔrɔ na ɩka ba nyɔɔ wʋ tɩchɛ nɩrɛ jaa ba 'la sɩɩr wʋ nɩ wʋ nũu ɛ.
43007045	A puorfʋ yir gugurbo lɩɛb chen a Farasee nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃, ka ba sʋʋr ba, "Ŋmɩnɛ wʋ ɩ ka yaa waan wʋ ɛ?"
43007046	Ka a bala ban tʋ̃, ka ba 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ jaa ba 'yɛr 'yɛr a daba nyã kaar ɛ."
43007047	Ka a Faraseemɩne sʋʋr ba, "Wʋ mɩ ben bɛl yɩ wɛ?
43007048	Yɩ nyɛn a Faraseemɩne nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ ka ba sɔɔ de wʋ?
43007049	Kai, tɩchɛ a nɩyɔɔ ba nyãna ba bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ ɛ, ba ben pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ gba."
43007050	Nikodimasɩ na dɔ̃ɔ chen a Yesu sɛ̃ mɩ ɩ naa a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ sʋʋr ba,
43007051	"A nɛɛ ba kʋ sɩ sɔr ɩka sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ yele ka saa wõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr bɩɩ maala ɛ?"
43007052	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ mɩ yin Galilee bɩɩ? Jʋʋr kaa, a la ɩ fʋ nyɛn Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ na yi Galilee."
43007053	Ka ba jaa yaar kul a ba yie.
43008001	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu mɩ do a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ ju.
43008002	Wɛr na wa chaar bibio pipi, Yesu lɩɛb wa kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, be lɛ a nɩbɛ ŋmaa jilʋ̃ wʋ tɩ wʋ jɩ̃nɛ wile ba.
43008003	Be lɛ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwiilbe, nɩ a Faraseemɩne wa 'mataa waan pɔɔ ban nyɔɔ na gãn daba. Ba vɛ̃n ka a pɔɔ ir ara a ba jaa niem,
43008004	tɩ ba 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "Wiwile, a pɔɔ nyãna lɛ gãn daba ka sɩ nyɔɔ.
43008005	A Mosesɩ Nɛɛ 'lɔ 'yɛr ɩka sɩ lɔb wʋ nɩ kʋsɩɛ kʋ."
43008006	Ba 'yɛr naa a lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bɛɛr Yesu kaa na ba tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ 'yɛr, 'yɛr a wʋ yele. Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu guun de a nubir sɛɛrɛ nɩ a tẽe.
43008007	Tɩ ba chɛnɛ sʋrɔ wʋ, ka wʋ dɔl 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ben ka ba maal dɛɛr ɛ, a nɩnyɩnɛ wʋ de nie lɔb a pɔɔ nɩ a kʋsɩr."
43008008	Tɩ na wʋ lɛ guun sɛɛrɛ a tẽe go.
43008009	A anyãna ban wõ, ba piel yire bʋ̃'yen 'yen, a danyɔ̃n lɛ de nie. A wa tɩ chɛ naa a Yesu nɩ a pɔɔ tɛɛ na ara a be.
43008010	Yesu dɔl ir sʋʋr a pɔɔ, "Nyɛ ba be? Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ yele ɛ?"
43008011	Ka a pɔɔ 'yɛr, "Kai nɩkpɛ̃ɛ." Ka Yesu mɩ pãa 'yɛr wʋ, "Maa mɩ kʋ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ yele ɛ, chiine, taa lɛ wa maala yeldɛɛr go ɛ."
43008012	Yesu lɛ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ a wɛr nyã chãa, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na turo ma kʋ̃ lɛ chen libe pɔ ɛ, tɩ wʋn tara na nyɛvʋr na ɩ chãa."
43008013	Ka a Faraseemɩne chɩrɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Fʋ bʋɔrɔ na yuor 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ fʋ mɩ̃ɛ, ka a fʋ yobɔ ɩ pɔrɔ."
43008014	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ n bʋɔrɔ naa yuor 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a n mɩ̃ɛ, a n yobɔ tara na sɔr. Bojũu n bɔ̃ɔ naa jie ɩn yi wa, naa lɛ bɔ̃ɔ a jie ɩn chiine. Tɩchɛ yɩn, yaa bɔ̃ɔ a jie ɩn yi wa ɛ, yaa lɛ bɔ̃ɔ a jie ɩn chiine ɛ.
43008015	Yɩ den nɩsaal tɩɛrsɩ tɔɔrɔ nɩ 'yɛr, maa ba tɔɔrɔ nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr ɛ.
43008016	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ ɩn tɔɔr naa 'yɛr, a lɛ ɩn na tɔɔr na tor naa bojũu n ba ɩ n yõ ɛ, a Sãa na tʋ̃ ma pʋɔ ma naa.
43008017	A sɛb a yɩ nɛɛr pɔ ɩka, nɩbɛ ayi 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43008018	N 'yɛrɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a n mɩ̃ɛ, ka a Sãa mɩ na tʋ̃ ma 'yɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma."
43008019	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Nyɩnɛ a fʋ Sãa be?" Ka Yesu 'yɛr "Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ma ɛ, bɩɩ a n Sãa ɛ, ala ɩ yɩ ta bɔ̃ɔ ma naa, yɩn taa bɔ̃ɔ naa n Sãa mɩ."
43008020	Yesu 'yɛr naa a 'yɛr nyã wʋn wile ba a puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ gbʋr a libie lɔb fʋ jie. Tɩ nɩrɛ jaa ba nyɔɔ wʋ ɛ, an ɩ a wʋ bɩbir ba vɩɛ ɛ.
43008021	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba go, "N chiine na, yɩn wa yʋɔrɔ na bʋɔrɔ ma tɩ na yɩ kpin a yɩ yelbier. Jie ɩn chiine, yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wa be ɛ."
43008022	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ pãa sʋrɔ taa, "Wʋn kʋn wʋ mɩ̃ɛ bɩɩ? Ala lɛ so wʋn 'yɛr ɩka, 'A jie ɩn chiine yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wa be ɛ.' "
43008023	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩn yin ka tẽe, maa yin saaju. A wɛr nyã pɔ lɛ yɩ yi, maa mɩ ba yi a wɛr nyã pɔ ɛ.
43008024	N 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka yɩn kpin naa yɩ yelbier, ala ɩ yaa sɔɔ de ma nɩ a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr ɩka n ɩ naa ɛ, sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, yɩn kpin naa yɩ yelbier."
43008025	Ka a nɩbɛ sʋʋr wʋ, "An fʋ ɩ?" A Yesu 'yɛr ba, "N ɩ naa a 'lɔ ɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a kõr jaa.
43008026	N tara na yɔɔ ɩn taa 'yɛr tɔɔr a yɩ 'yɛr, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, ala ɩn wõ yi a wʋ sɛ̃ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a wɛr nɩbɛ."
43008027	Baa bɔ̃ɔ a par ɩka a wʋ Sãa 'yɛr lɛ wʋ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ ɛ.
43008028	Be a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩn wa 'mɔɔ a Nɩsaal Bie a saaju yɩn bɔ̃ɔ naa a nɩrɛ 'lɔ ɩn ɩ, na yɩ mɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka n ba ɩrɛ yele nɩ maa kpɛ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ naa a lɛ a Sãa na wiil ma.
43008029	A 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma be naa n sɛ̃, waa bar ma n yõ ɛ, bojũu n ma ɩrɛ naa lɛ na pɛlɛ a wʋ pʋɔ."
43008030	Wʋn 'yɛrɛ a lɛ tɩ nɩyɔɔ sɔɔn de wʋ.
43008031	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bala na sɔɔ de wʋ, "Ala ɩ yɩ sɔɔn turo a lɛ ɩn wiil yɩ, yɩn ɩ naa a n poturbo yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43008032	Yɩn bɔ̃ɔn a yelmɩ̃ɛ, ka a yelmɩ̃ɛ for yɩ bar ka yɩ so yɩ mɩ̃ɛ."
43008033	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Sɩn ɩ naa Abraham yɔn, na saa ɩ nɩrɛ jaa gbãgbaar ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ fʋ 'yɛr ɩka ban for sɩn bar ka sɩ so sɩ mɩ̃ɛ?"
43008034	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ jaa na maal dɛɛr ɩn a dɛɛr gbãgbaa.
43008035	Gbãgbaa maa be a yir kor ɛ, a bie 'lɔ ma ben be kor.
43008036	Ala wa ɩ a Bie for fʋn bar, fʋn son fʋ mɩ sɩrɛ jaa.
43008037	N bɔ̃ɔn na yɩn ɩ Abraham yɔn tɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ kʋ ma, bojũu yaa sɔɔ a n 'yɛr ɛ.
43008038	Maa 'yɛrɛ yɩ naa a lɛ ɩn nyɛ a n Sãa sɛ̃, ka yɩn mɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ yɩn wõ a yɩ sãa sɛ̃."
43008039	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Abraham lɛ ɩ a sɩ sãa." Be a Yesu 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ Abraham bibiir lɛ yɩ ta ɩ, yɩn taa maal a lɛ a Abraham na dɔ̃ɔ maal.
43008040	Yɩ ben bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ kʋ ma a nɩrɛ na 'yɛr yɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩn wõ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃. Abraham ba dɔ̃ɔ maal lɛ ɛ.
43008041	Yɩ ɩrɛ naa a lɛ a yɩ sãa mɩ̃ɛ na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ." Ka ba 'yɛr, "Saa ɩ sɛ̃sɛ̃ bibiir ɛ, sɩn Sãa tɛɛ sɩn tara lɛ Nãaŋmɩn."
43008042	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ta ɩ a yɩ Sãa, yɩn taa nʋ̃ ma naa. Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ lɛ n yi naa be be ka a pʋ̃pãanyã. N ba waan a n mɩ̃ɛ yuor ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ tʋ̃ ma.
43008043	Bo lɛ so ka a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr ba chaar kʋ yɩ ɛ? Bojũu yaa tʋ̃ɔ wõ a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr ɛ.
43008044	A yɩ sãa ɩn tɩɩ, a yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ maal a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ. An yi a pielfʋ jaa nɩkʋrɔ lɛ wʋ ɩ, waa tara yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, yelmɩ̃ɛ bɩ̃lãa jaa ba be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ. 'Lɔ wa ŋmaara a jire, lɛ wʋ be, jir ŋmara lɛ wʋ ɩ, na wʋ ɩ a jie a jaa sãa.
43008045	Tɩchɛ maa na 'yɛrɛ a yelmɩ̃ɛ yaa sɔɔ de ma ɛ.
43008046	A yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na 'yɛr ɩka wʋ nyɛn ɩn maal dɛɛr ɔ? Ala ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ, bo lɛ so ka yaa sɔɔ de ma ɛ?
43008047	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn tʋɔr wõnõ naa a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ. Yɩn ba ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tʋɔr ɛ, yaa wõnõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ ɛ."
43008048	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ sɩ 'yɛrɛ ɩka Samariya lɛ fʋ yi na fʋ tara a sɩdɛɛr."
43008049	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Maa ba sɩdɛɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ n 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ naa a n Sãa, tɩ yɩn ba 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma ɛ.
43008050	N ba bʋɔrɔ tɩɩr kʋrɔ a n mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ bʋɔrɔ naa a lɛ. 'Lɔ Lɛ ɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ.
43008051	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ala ɩ nɩrɛ turo naa maa 'yɛr, wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ kũu ɛ."
43008052	A anyãna lɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ pãa 'yɛrɛ, "Pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa fʋn tara a sɩdɛɛr. Abraham kpi naa, ka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ kpi, tɩchɛ ka fʋ 'yɛr ɩka ala ɩ nɩrɛ turo naa a fʋ 'yɛr wʋ kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔ kũu ɛ.
43008053	Fʋ̃ʋ bɛrma gar a sɩ sãa Abraham bɩɩ? Wʋ kpi naa, ka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ mɩ kpi. An fʋ tɩɛr ɩka fʋ pãa ɩ naa?"
43008054	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ n ben 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a n mɩ̃ɛ tɩɩr, a n tɩɩr na ɩn pɔrɔ. A n Sãa 'lɔ yɩn 'yɛrɛ ɩka a yɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ, 'lɔ lɛ kʋrɔ ma a tɩɩr.
43008055	Yɩn ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ gba ɛ, maa bɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa. Ala ɩ n 'yɛr naa ɩka n ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ, ɩn ɩ naa jir ŋmara a yɩ kaar. Tɩchɛ maa bɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa, naa turo a wʋ 'yɛr bie.
43008056	A yɩ sãa Abraham dɔ̃ɔ chɩlɛ tɩɛr ɩka wʋn taa nyɛ naa a n bɩbir. Wʋ nyɛn ka nʋ̃ɔ nyɔɔ wʋ."
43008057	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ sʋʋr wʋ, "Faa ta yuom lɩjaayi nɩ pie (50) sɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ na fʋ nyɛ Abraham?"
43008058	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, sɛrɛ tɩ ba wa dɔɔ Abraham, ka maa dɔ̃ɔ be be."
43008059	A nyãna, ka ba wob kʋsɩbɛ ɩka ba lɔb wʋ kʋ, tɩchɛ ka a Yesu sɔɔl fʋɔl na wʋ yi a be a ba puorfʋ yir pɔ.
43009001	Yesu na chiine a lɛ, wʋ nyɛn daba ban dɔɔ ka wʋ ɩ jɔ̃ɔ.
43009002	Ka a poturbo sʋʋr wʋ, "Wiwile, an lɛ maal dɛɛr, a dajɔ̃ɔ bɩɩ a wʋ sãa naa ma lɛ maal dɛɛr, a dajɔ̃ɔ bɩɩ a wʋ sãa naa ma lɛ maal a dɛɛr dɔɔn wʋ, ka wʋ ɩ a jɔ̃ɔ?"
43009003	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A daba nyã ba maal dɛɛr ɛ, a wʋ sãa naa ma mɩ ba maal dɛɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ a ɩn a lɛ ka Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃mɔ̃ na tʋ̃ a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43009004	An chɛnɛ ɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ, sɩn tʋ̃ naa a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma tʋ̃mɔ̃. Wɛr na sɔb naa ka nɩrɛ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃mɔ̃ tʋ̃ ɛ.
43009005	Ɩn chɛnɛ be a wɛr pɔ, maa lɛ a wɛr chãa."
43009006	Wʋn wa 'yɛr a lɛ baar, wʋ chir nataar bun tãn a tẽe na wʋ bɛ a daba nɩbie.
43009007	Tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a daba, "Chen, tɩ pɛɛ a Siloam kʋ̃ɔ pɔ." A Siloam par lɛ, Tʋ̃fʋ. Wʋ chen tɩ pɛɛ nyɛrɛ wa a yir.
43009008	Ka a nɩbɔ̃ɔnsɩ bala na dɔ̃ɔ ma nyɛ wʋ na sʋɔrɔ, ka ba sʋrɔ taa, "A ba ɩ a daba nyãna lɛ ma sʋɔrɔ ɛ?"
43009009	Bamɩne 'yɛr ɩka 'lɔ lɛ, ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr, "Nɩnyɛtaa lɛ." Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ."
43009010	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Ŋmɩnɛ a nɩbie ɩrɛ wa yuo fʋ?"
43009011	Ka a daba 'yɛr kʋ ba. "Daba ban bʋɔlɔ Yesu lɛ bu tãn bɛ ma a nɩbie tɩ 'yɛr ma ɩka n chen a Siloam tɩ pɛɛ. Lɛ lɛ n chen tɩ pɛɛ naa nyɛrɛ."
43009012	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ wʋ be?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "N ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ."
43009013	Be lɛ ba tara a daba 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a jɔ̃ɔ chiin a Faraseemɩne sɛ̃.
43009014	A bɩbir 'lɔ a Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ bu a tãn na wʋ yuon a daba nɩbie ɩn a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar.
43009015	Ka Faraseemɩne sʋʋr a daba lɛ wʋn ɩrɛ wa nyɛrɛ. Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Tãn lɛ wʋ bɛ ma a nɩbie ka n pɛɛ be nyɛrɛ."
43009016	Ka a Faraseemɩne bamɩne 'yɛr, "A daba nyã ba yi Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ, waa sɔ̃nɔ̃ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir ɛ." Tɩchɛ ka a bamɩne mɩ sʋʋr, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ yelbe-ɩrɛ na tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ a nɛ'maa yele nyã?" Na ba ŋma jiir ayi.
43009017	Ka ba lɩɛb sʋʋr a daba, "Bo fʋ tara na 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr? Fʋ nɩbie ba lɛ wʋ yuo." Ka a daba 'yɛr, "Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ."
43009018	Ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ ba sɔɔ de ɛ ɩka a daba dɔ̃ɔ jɔ̃ɔ tɩ wa nyɛrɛ ɛ, ka ba bʋɔl a sãa naa ma.
43009019	Ba sʋʋr ba naa, "A yɩ bie lɛ a nyã ɔ? A nyã lɛ yɩ dɔɔ ka wʋ ɩ a jɔ̃ɔ? Ka ŋmɩnɛ wʋ ɩrɛ wa nyɛrɛ?"
43009020	Ka a sãa naa ma 'yɛr, "Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka sɩ bie lɛ, a sɩ dɔɔ wʋ ka wʋ ɩ jɔ̃ɔ.
43009021	Tɩchɛ lɛ wʋn ɩrɛ wa nyɛrɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã saa bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, bɩɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na yuo wʋ a nɩbie saa bɔ̃ɔ ɛ. Waa ɩ bibile ɛ, yɩ sʋʋr wʋ, wʋn 'yɛr kʋ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ."
43009022	A sãa naa ma 'yɛr naa nɩtɔ̃ bojũu ba joro naa a Juu nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ, ba den nie 'yɛr ɩka nɩrɛ jaa wa 'yɛr ɩka a Yesu lɛ a Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ, ka ban dii wʋn bar a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie.
43009023	Ala lɛ so ka a sãa naa ma 'yɛr, "Waa ɩ bibile ɛ, yɩ sʋʋr wʋ."
43009024	A Faraseemɩne lɛ bʋɔl naa a daba 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a jɔ̃ɔ a gbɛɛ ayi sʋɔ 'yɛr wʋ, "'Yɛr yelmɩ̃ɛ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, sɩn bɔ̃ɔn naa a daba nyã na ɩ yelbe-ɩrɛ."
43009025	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ wʋ ɩn yelbe-ɩrɛ bɩɩ waa ɩ ɛ, n ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, yelbʋ̃'yen ɩn bɔ̃ɔ nɩ nyã. N dɔ̃ɔ ɩ jɔ̃ɔ tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, n nyɛrɛ naa."
43009026	Be lɛ ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Bo lɛ wʋ ɩ fʋ? Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ yuo fʋ a nɩbie?"
43009027	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "N ba dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr tɩ yaa chɛlɛ ɛ. Bo yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ lɛ wõ ka a ɩ go? Yɩ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ mɩ lɩɛb a wʋ poturbo bɩɩ?"
43009028	A ba tʋrɔ wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a wʋ poturo, sɩn ɩ naa Mosesɩ poturbo.
43009029	Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn na ɩka Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ Mosesɩ, tɩchɛ a daba 'lɔ saa bɔ̃ɔ jie wʋn yi gba ɛ."
43009030	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "A 'maa man nɛɛ yɩn ba bɔ̃ɔ jie wʋn yi ɛ, tɩ yuo ma a nɩbie.
43009031	Sɩ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn ba chɛlɛ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ ɛ. Wʋ ma chɛlɛ naa a bala na joro wʋ tɩ maala a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ.
43009032	Nɩrɛ jaa ba dɔ̃ɔ wõ ɩka ba yuon nɩrɛ ban lɔ̃ɔ dɔɔn jɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
43009033	Ala ɩ a daba nyã ba ta yi Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ naa tʋ̃ɔ bon jaa maal ɛ."
43009034	Ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ 'yɛr kʋ a daba, "A fʋ̃ʋ, yelbier pɔ lɛ ba dɔɔ fʋ, ŋmɩnɛ fʋn ɩrɛ wa wiil sɩ," tɩ dii wʋ bar a ba pɔ.
43009035	Yesu na wõ ɩka ba dii naa a daba bar, wʋ bɔ wʋn wa nyɛ wʋ, na wʋ sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ sɔɔn de a Nɩsaal Bie ɔ?"
43009036	Ka a daba sʋʋr wʋ, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ an lɛ, wiil ma ka n sɔɔ de wʋ."
43009037	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Fʋ nyɛ wʋ naa pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩrɛ jaa, 'lɔ lɛ 'yɛrɛ nɩ fʋ."
43009038	Ka a daba pãa 'yɛr, "N Soro n sɔɔn de," tɩ gbur dumo puor wʋ.
43009039	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr, "'Yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie lɛ n wa ka a wɛr pɔ. Jɔ̃n na nyɛrɛ naa ka nɩbinyɛrɛ mɩ lɩɛb ɩ jɔ̃n."
43009040	Ka a Faraseemɩne bamɩne na be a wʋ sɛ̃ wõ a lɛ na ba sʋʋr, "Bo ya! A sɩn mɩ ɩn a jɔ̃n ɔ?"
43009041	A Yesu 'yɛr ba, "Ala ɩ yɩ ta ɩn jɔ̃n, yɩ kʋ naa tara chɛfʋ a dɛɛr pɔ ɛ. Tɩchɛ, yɩn ben 'yɛr ɩka yɩ nyɛrɛ naa, yɩ chɛnɛ na be a yɩ dɛɛr pɔ."
43010001	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na maa tu a piir jɔɔ dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ tɩ do a dachin kpɛ, ɩn nãnyie nɩ nɩfara.
43010002	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tu a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ kpɛ 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a pɛchinɛ.
43010003	A dɔ̃dɔ̃guro ma yuon a pãn kʋ a pɛchinɛ, ka a piir chɛlɛ a wʋ kɔkɔr. Wʋ maa bʋɔl naa a wʋ piir yoe, na wʋ ŋmaa ba yin.
43010004	'Lɔ wa ŋmaa a wʋ piir a jaa ka a yi, wʋ ma den nie ka a turo wʋ, bojũu ba bɔ̃ɔ naa a wʋ kɔkɔr.
43010005	Tɩchɛ ba kʋ̃ wa tu sãan jaa ɛ, ban jon yi a wʋ sɛ̃ bojũu baa bɔ̃ɔ sãan kɔkɔr ɛ."
43010006	Yesu lɔb a sʋkpa nyã tɩchɛ baa bɔ̃ɔ a par a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ ba ɛ.
43010007	A lɛ jũu lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr ba go, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, maa lɛ a piir dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ.
43010008	A bala ba jaa na dɔ̃ɔ ma nie wa ɩn nãnyisɩ nɩ nɩfarba, tɩchɛ a piir ba chɛlɛ ba ɛ.
43010009	Maa lɛ a dɔ̃dɔr, nɩrɛ jaa na tu ma kpɛ, wʋn nyɛn faafʋ. Wʋn ma kpɛ̃n tɩ yi na wʋ nyɛrɛ bʋ̃diir.
43010010	Nãnyie ma wa naa ɩka wʋ wa ju, na wʋ kʋ, tɩ sɔ̃ɔ bar. Maa wa naa ka ban nyɛ nyɛvʋr, na ba nyɛ wʋ tɩ põn bar.
43010011	"Maa lɛ a pɛchiin sʋ̃, a pɛchiin sʋ̃ sɔɔn kpi a wʋ piir 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43010012	A pɛchinɛ 'lɔ ban yara, waa so a piir ɛ. 'Lɔ wa nyɛ gbõgboro na waara, wʋ ma tɛɛn a piir bar tɩ jo, ka a gbõgboro yɛ̃yɛl a piir tɩ nyɔɔr amɩne.
43010013	Wʋ ma jon a lɛ an ɩ libie tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃, a piir yele ba bã wʋ ɛ.
43010014	"Maa ɩ naa a pɛchiin sʋ̃, n bɔ̃ɔ naa a n piir, ka n piir mɩ bɔ̃ɔ ma.
43010015	Nɩtãa lɛ a Sãa na bɔ̃ɔ ma ka n mɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Sãa, ɩn sɔɔn kpi a piir 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43010016	N tara na piir amɩne na ba be a jɔɔ nyã pɔ ɛ, ɩn waan ba naa, ka ba mɩ wa chɛlɛ a n kɔkɔr, ka ba ɩ pɛgbul bʋ̃'yen na ba tara pɛchiin bʋ̃'yen.
43010017	A n Sãa na nʋ̃ ma par nɩ nyã, n sɔɔ naa na kpi tɩ lɛ ir ɩ vʋr go.
43010018	Nɩrɛ baa faara wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ maa mɩ̃ɛ lɛ sɔɔ na kpi. N tara na kpɛ̃ɔ na bar a nyɛvʋr naa lɛ tara kpɛ̃ɔ na de wʋ go. A nyã lɛ a n Sãa 'yɛr ma ɩka n ɩ."
43010019	A 'yɛr nyã lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Juu nɩbɛ ŋma dẽ dẽ.
43010020	Ka a ba yɔɔ 'yɛrɛ ɩka, "Sɩdɛɛr lɛ wʋ tara, na wʋ gele, bo 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ chɛlɛ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ?"
43010021	Tɩchɛ ka a bamɩne 'yɛrɛ, "A nyãna ba ɩ nɩrɛ na tara sɩdɛɛr 'yɛr ɛ, a sɩdɛɛr na tʋ̃ɔn yuo jɔ̃ɔ nɩbie ɔ?"
43010022	A ɩ naa uon ka ba maala a ba puorfʋ yir Pɔlfʋ lɔ̃ɔ di be a Jerusalɛm.
43010023	Ka Yesu be be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, na wʋ yʋɔrɔ a be ban bʋɔlɔ a Solomon Jɛ̃bɛr.
43010024	Be a Juu nɩbɛrɛ bamɩne ŋmaa jilʋ̃ wʋ sʋrɔ, "A baalfʋ nyã fʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ, dabor an wa baar? Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa 'lɔ, 'yɛr kʋ sɩ chãa pɔ."
43010025	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "N dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr yɩ, yɩn lɛ ba sɔɔ de ɛ. A nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɩn tʋ̃ nɩ a n Sãa yuor, 'yɛr naa n 'yɛr.
43010026	Tɩchɛ yɩn lɛ ba sɔɔ de ɛ, bojũu yaa ɩ a n piir ɛ.
43010027	A n piir ma chɛlɛ naa a n kɔkɔr, n bɔ̃ɔ ba naa ka ba ma turo ma.
43010028	N kʋ ban nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. Ba kʋ̃ wɛ ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ba 'loo faa a n nũu pɔ ɛ.
43010029	A n Sãa 'lɔ na de ba kʋ ma, wʋ gar bomo a jaa. Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ba 'loo faa a n Sãa nũu pɔ ɛ.
43010030	Maa naa n Sãa jaa ɩn bʋ̃'yen."
43010031	Ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ wob kʋsɩbɛ ɩka ba lɔb wʋ go.
43010032	Tɩchɛ ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "N tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃yɔɔ yi a Sãa sɛ̃, buor sʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ pãa be lɔɔrɔ ma?"
43010033	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Saa lɔɔrɔ fʋ a anyã ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ fʋn fere sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn yuor, tɩ mɩ ɩ nɩsaal."
43010034	A Yesu 'yɛr ba, "A ba sɛb a yɩ Nɛɛ pɔ ɩka, 'N 'yɛr naa ɩka, yɩ ɩn ŋmɩmɛ ɛ?'
43010035	Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl naa a bala a wʋ 'yɛr, na wa a ba sɛ̃, ŋmɩmɛ, Nãaŋmɩn sɛɛr ba be na wa sɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
43010036	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a 'lɔ a Sãa na kaa ir a wʋ bɔfʋ pɔ, na wʋ tʋ̃ ka a wɛr pɔ. Bo lɛ so ka yaa bara ma ɛ, bojũu n 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn Bie lɛ n ɩ?
43010037	Yɩ taa sɔɔ de ma ɛ, ala ɩ n ba maala a lɛ a Sãa na maala ɛ.
43010038	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ n tʋ̃ naa, yɩn gba ba sɔɔ de ma ɛ, yɩ sɔɔ de a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃, yɩn bɔ̃ɔn a par ɩka a Sãa ben a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ka n mɩ be a Sãa 'yɔ̃ɔ."
43010039	Ka ba lɛ bʋɔrɔ a wʋ nyɔɔfʋ go, tɩ chɛ ka wʋ fʋɔl yi.
43010040	Be lɛ a Yesu lɩɛb gɔ̃ɔ a Jordan man gɔ̃ɔn, a jie 'lɔ a Jɔɔn na dɔ̃ɔ suoro a nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ na wʋ jɛ̃ a be,
43010041	ka nɩyɔɔ wa a wʋ sɛ̃ wa 'yɛrɛ, "Jɔɔn gba ba dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃ nɛ 'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ, a ala a jaa wʋn 'yɛr a daba nyã 'yɛr, ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ."
43010042	Be lɛ a nɩyɔɔ sɔɔ de wʋ.
43011001	Daba ban bʋɔlɔ Lajarusɩ dɔ̃ɔ bɩɛrɛ, wʋ ɩn Mɛɛr nɩ Mata yɛdaba na ba kpɩɛrɛ a Betanɩ tẽe pɔ.
43011002	A Mɛɛr nyã na dɔ̃ɔ kpaar a kãnyũu 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu tɩ de a wʋ jukɔɔl fɩɛl, a wʋ yɛdaba Lajarusɩ lɛ a nyã na bɩɛrɛ.
43011003	Ka a yɛpɔbɔ tʋ̃ 'yɛr a Yesu, "Sɩ Soro, a fʋ baraa bɩɛrɛ naa."
43011004	Yesu na wõ a lɛ, a wʋ 'yɛr, "A baal nyã ba ɩ kũu baal ɛ, tɩ an wiil Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr tɩ mɩ vɛ̃ ka Nãaŋmɩn Bie yuor yi."
43011005	Yesu nʋ̃n Mata nɩ a wʋ yɛbɛ nɩ a ba yɛdaba Lajarusɩ.
43011006	Tɩchɛ wʋn wõ a Lajarusɩ baal tɩ na wʋ chɛnɛ jɩ̃nɛ a be wʋn be ber ayi.
43011007	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ poturbo, "Yɩ ɩ a sɩ lɩɛb chen a Judiya."
43011008	Tɩchɛ ka a poturbo 'yɛr, "Wiwile, daar yɛ̃ yɛ̃ nyãna ba lɛ a Juu nɩbɛrɛ ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba lɔb fʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a fʋ lɛ chiine a be go?"
43011009	Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A ba ɩ a bɩbir tara na a wʋ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ chaarfʋ sɔ̃ɔ ɛ? Nɩrɛ wa chiine a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ wʋ maa ŋme gbɛr ɛ, wʋ nyɛ naa a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ chãa.
43011010	Bojũu ala ɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ lɛ wʋ chiine, wʋn ŋmen gbɛr, bojũu waa tara chãa ɛ."
43011011	Wʋn wa 'yɛr a lɛ baar, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A sɩ baraa Lajarusɩ gur naa, tɩchɛ ɩn chen tɩ sɩ̃ɩ wʋ."
43011012	Ka a wʋ poturbo 'yɛr, "Sɩ Soro, ala ɩ wʋ gur naa, wʋn ir naa."
43011013	Yesu 'lɔ 'yɛr naa ɩka wʋ kpi naa, tɩchɛ ka a poturbo 'lɔ tɩɛr ɩka a gʋ̃ɔ sʋ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ.
43011014	Ala lɛ so a Yesu pãa 'yɛr ka a chaar ɩka, "Lajarusɩ kpi naa.
43011015	A yɩ jũu, a nʋ̃mɔ̃ ma naa ɩn ba be be ɛ, ka yɩ na sɔɔ de ma. Tɩchɛ, yɩ ɩ a sɩ chen a wʋ sɛ̃."
43011016	A wʋ poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Tomasɩ na ba lɛ bʋɔlɔ wʋ Naa 'yɛr kʋ a bala na chɛ, "Yɩ ɩ a sɩ 'mataa chiin wʋ mɩ tɩ kpi."
43011017	Yesu na wa ta a be, wʋ nyɛn ka a ɩ ba ũu naa Lajarusɩ maal ber anaar.
43011018	Betanɩ nɩ a Jerusalɛm mɩ ba jãa ɛ.
43011019	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ yɔɔ chen ɩka ba tɩ puor a Mata nɩ a Mɛɛr a ba yɛdaba kuor.
43011020	Mata na wa wõ ɩka Yesu waara naa, wʋ yin tɩ tuor wʋ, tɩchɛ kaa Mɛɛr 'lɔ jɩ̃nɛ a yir.
43011021	Be lɛ a Mata 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "N Soro, fʋ̃ʋ ta dɔ̃ɔ be ka, a n yɛdaba kʋ̃ naa kpi ɛ.
43011022	Tɩchɛ n bɔ̃ɔ naa pʋ̃pãanyã gba ɩka, bon jaa fʋn sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, wʋn kʋ fʋ naa."
43011023	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A fʋ yɛdaba na ir naa a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋr."
43011024	Be lɛ a Mata 'yɛr kʋ a Yesu, "N bɔ̃ɔn na wʋn na ir a kũn irfʋ daar, a ber baaraa sɔ̃ɔ."
43011025	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Maa lɛ ɩ a kũu pɔ irfʋ, nɩ nyɛvʋr, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔɔ de ma, 'lɔ kpi gba, tɩ wʋn tara na nyɛvʋr.
43011026	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba kpi ɛ, tɩ na wʋ sɔɔ de ma, kʋ̃ lɛ kpi ɛ, fʋ sɔɔ naa a lɛ ɔ?"
43011027	Ka a Mata 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, n Soro, n sɔɔn de ɩka fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn Bie, 'lɔn na wa ka a wɛr pɔ."
43011028	Wʋn wa 'yɛr a lɛ baar wʋ lɩɛb kul tɩ bʋl 'yɛr kʋ a yɛbile Mɛɛr, "A wiwile ben ka tɩ sʋrɔ fʋ."
43011029	A Mɛɛr na wa wõ a lɛ, ka wʋ vaa ir chen a Yesu sɛ̃.
43011030	Yesu ba kpɛ a tẽe pɔ sɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ chɛnɛ ara a be a Mata na tuor wʋ.
43011031	A Juu nɩbɛ bala na wa a kuor puorfʋ jie be a Mɛɛr sɛ̃ a yir, na nyɛ a lɛ wʋn vaa ir yire, ka ba turo wʋ tɩɛr ɩka a yaa par lɛ wʋ chiine a kõn jie.
43011032	Mɛɛr na tɩ ta a jie nyɛ a Yesu a be, wʋ gbur dumo a Yesu niem tɩ 'yɛr, "N Soro, fʋ̃ʋ ta dɔ̃ɔ be ka, a n yɛdaba kʋ̃ naa kpi ɛ."
43011033	Yesu na nyɛ a lɛ wʋn kõnõ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bala na bɩɛl wʋ mɩ kõnõ, nɩbaal kpɛ wʋ naa ka a suur nyɔɔ wʋ.
43011034	A wʋ sʋʋr ba, "Nyɩnɛ yɩ ũu wʋ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "N Soro, wa nyɛ a jie."
43011035	Ka Yesu kõ.
43011036	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ pãa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Nyɛ lɛ wʋn nʋ̃ a Lajarusɩ."
43011037	Tɩchɛ ka bamɩne pãa 'yɛr, "Wʋn dɔ̃ɔ yuo a jɔ̃ɔ nɩbie, kaa ɩ wʋ kʋ̃ naa tʋ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka a Lajarusɩ ta kpi bɩɩ?"
43011038	Ka nɩbaal kpɛ a Yesu, ka wʋ tɔɔ ta a yaa par. Kʋsɩr bɔɔ lɛ, ka ba 'mɔɔ a kʋsɩr ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔɔ a nɛɛ.
43011039	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Yɩ bil a kʋsɩr bar." Tɩchɛ a Mata an ɩ a wʋ yɛdaba lɛ kpi, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "N Soro, wʋn nyuro naa, ber anaar nɩ dɩna ban ũu wʋ."
43011040	Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "N ba 'yɛr fʋ ɩka fʋ̃ʋ sɔɔ de, fʋn nyɛn Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr ɛ?"
43011041	Be lɛ ba bil a kʋsɩr bar, a Yesu kaa saaju tɩ 'yɛr, "N Sãa, fʋ son puorfʋ, fʋn wõ a n sʋɔrfʋ.
43011042	N bɔ̃ɔn naa fʋn wõnõ a n sʋɔrfʋ, tɩchɛ n 'yɛr naa ka a na sʋ̃ʋ a nɩbɛ banyãna na ara a ka, a ba sɔɔ de ɩka, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ tʋ̃ ma."
43011043	Yesu na 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ wʋ bʋɔl kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, "Lajarusɩ, wa yi."
43011044	Ka a kũu yi, ka a gbɛɛ naa nuur ban vil a fɔpɩɛl pɔɔ ka a fɔbaa mɩ pɔɔ a ju. A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ yaar a kũu fɔɔr bar wʋ ka wʋ chen."
43011045	Ala lɛ so ka a Juu nɩbɛ bala na wa ɩka ba wa puor a Mɛɛr, nyɛn a lɛ a Yesu na ɩ, a ba sɔɔ wʋ.
43011046	Tɩchɛ ka a bamɩne chen a Faraseemɩne sɛ̃ tɩ man a lɛ a Yesu na maal.
43011047	Be lɛ a Faraseemɩne nɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ bʋɔl taa lɔ̃ɔfʋ na ba 'yɛr, "Ŋmɩnɛ sɩn ɩ, a daba nyã na ben tʋ̃nɔ̃ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ a nɩtɔ̃?
43011048	Ala ɩ sɩn be bar wʋ ka wʋ maala lɛ, nɩrɛ jaa na sɔɔn a wʋ yele, a Worom nɩbɛ wa wõ a yele ban wa wɛl sɩ naa a jisʋ̃ nɩ a tẽe bar."
43011049	Ka a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Kayafasɩ na ɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a yuon 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ 'yɛr, "Yaa tara tɩɛr jaa ɛ.
43011050	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a sɛɛ naa ka nɩbʋ̃'yen na kpi kʋ a nɩyɔɔ gar a nɩyɔɔ ba jaa na wɛ ɛ."
43011051	A nyã ba yi a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ sɛ̃ ka wʋ 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋn ɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a yuon 'lɔ, ala lɛ wʋ de nie dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩka a Yesu na kpin kʋ a Juu nɩbʋrɔ ba jaa.
43011052	A ba ɩ bala tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ lɔ̃ɔ taa a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir bala na yɛ̃yɛl na wʋ maal ba a ba ɩ bʋ̃'yen.
43011053	An yi a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ba bʋɔrɔ na sɔr na kʋ a Yesu.
43011054	A lɛ juu Yesu ba lɛ yʋɔrɔ chãa pɔ a Juu nɩbɛ jie ɛ, tɩ chen jiyuo na gbʋr a mɔgɔ̃ɔ na wʋ tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a tẽbile ban bʋɔlɔ Eferɛm, be lɛ wʋ tɩ 'mataa jɛ̃n a wʋ poturbo.
43011055	A Juu nɩbɛ Gõl Bar Difʋ gbʋr naa, ka ba yɔɔ yi a tẽbil do a Jerusalɛm tɩ pɔlɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ chɛlɛ nɩ a bɩbir.
43011056	Ba kaara na bʋɔrɔ a Yesu a be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir, sʋrɔ taa, "Ŋmɩnɛ yɩ tɩɛr, wʋn wa naa a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie bɩɩ?"
43011057	Tɩchɛ ka a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Faraseemɩne 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ jaa wa bɔ̃ɔ a jie a Yesu na be, wʋ 'yɛr ka ba tɩ nyɔɔ wʋ."
43012001	A chɛn ber ayʋɔb ka a Gõl Bar Difʋ bɩbir ta. Yesu chen a Betanɩ na ɩ a Lajarusɩ 'lɔ na kpi ka wʋ sɩ̃ɩ kpɩɛrɛ.
43012002	Ba maal bʋ̃diir kʋ wʋ a be, ka a Mata põnõ a bʋ̃diir. Lajarusɩ pʋɔ naa a nɩbɛ bala na lɔ̃ɔ jɛ̃n Yesu a bʋ̃diir jie.
43012003	Be lɛ Mɛɛr de kãnyũu vɩla daa na ɩ tuo wa pʋr 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu gbɛɛ pɔ, tɩ lɩɛb a jukɔɔl fɩɛlɛ nɩ ka a nyũu de a yir wʋ jaa.
43012004	Tɩchɛ a wʋ poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Judas na yi a Isɩkariyot, 'lɔ lɛ na wa gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu sʋʋr,
43012005	"Bo lɛ so ka baa da a kãnyũu nyãna ɛ, a libie na tãn nɩrɛ yuon gbul sãyar na ba de kʋ nɔ̃n dẽme ɛ?"
43012006	A nɔ̃n dẽme yele ba bã wʋ ɛ, bojũu nãnyie lɛ wʋ ɩ an ɩ 'lɔ lɛ tara a ba libie wʋɔ, na wʋ ma juro a ala ban 'yɔ̃ɔ a be sʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
43012007	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Bar a pɔɔ jaa jomm, wʋ bin a kãnyũu nyãna gun a n ũufʋ bɩbir.
43012008	A nɔ̃n dẽme na ben a yɩ sɛ̃ bɩbir jaa, tɩchɛ maa kʋ̃ be a yɩ sɛ̃ bɩbir jaa ɛ."
43012009	A Juu yɔɔ jie na wõ ɩka Yesu be naa a Betanɩ, ba wa naa a ba ɩ a 'lɔ tɛɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ ba bʋɔrɔ na ɩka ba nyɛ a Lajarusɩ 'lɔ wʋn sɩ̃ɩ a kũu pɔ, ka wʋ ir ɩ vʋr.
43012010	A lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ, a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ mɩ guoro nɩ taa ɩka ba mɩn kʋ naa a Lajarusɩ.
43012011	A wʋ jũu lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ yɔɔ jie tɔr a ba nɩbɛrɛ wiilfʋ tɩ sɔɔrɔ a Yesu.
43012012	Wɛr na wa chaar, a nɩyɔɔ bala na wa a Gõl Bar Difʋ jie, wõ naa ɩka Yesu ben a sɔr pɔ waara a Jerusalɛm.
43012013	Ba 'mɛl bɛ vaɩ yi tuoro nɩ wʋ pãa chɩlɛ gɔ̃nɔ̃, "Yãan yooo, Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a 'lɔ wʋn tʋ̃. Nãaŋmɩn wʋ sʋ̃ʋ a 'lɔ na ɩ a Isɩral nãa."
43012014	Yesu nyɛn a bʋ̃pɔl na wʋ do jɩ̃nɛ nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ,
43012015	"A yɩn Jerusalɛm nɩbɛ, yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, Yɩ nyɛ a yɩ nãa na do bʋ̃pɔl waara nɩ."
43012016	A wʋ poturbo ba dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna a jaa par ɛ, tɩ a Yesu na wa ir ɩ vʋr, ba tɩɛr yuo ɩka anyãna lɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ka ba mɩ maal a lɛ kʋ wʋ.
43012017	A nɩyɔɔ bala na dɔ̃ɔ be a wʋ sɛ̃ na ba nyɛ a lɛ wʋn bʋɔl a Lajarusɩ ka wʋ yi a yaa pɔ ɩ vʋr, ba chɛnɛ na mana kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ.
43012018	Ala lɛ so ka a nɩyɔɔ yi tuoro wʋ, bojũu ba wõ naa ɩka wʋ tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃.
43012019	Be lɛ ka a Faraseemɩne pãa 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Yɩ nyɛ, saa lɛ tʋɔrɔ bon jaa maala ɛ. Nyɛ, a nɩbɛ ba jaa ben turo wʋ."
43012020	A nɩbɛ bamɩne mɩ na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, pʋɔ naa bala na do a puorfʋ jie a Jerusalɛm a Gõl Bar Difʋ sɔ̃ɔ.
43012021	Ba chen a Filip na yi a Betɩsaida na be a Galilee wɛr pɔ sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, sɩ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka sɩ nyɛ a Yesu."
43012022	Filip chen tɩ 'yɛr kʋ Andiru ka ba 'mataa chen tɩ 'yɛr a Yesu.
43012023	A Yesu 'yɛr ba, "A sɔ̃ɔ ta naa ka Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ a Nɩsaal Bie tɩɩr.
43012024	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, chibir baa ũu tẽe ɛ, wʋn chɛnɛ na ɩ a chibir bʋ̃'yen. Tɩchɛ 'lɔ wa lo tẽe kpi, wʋ ma dɔɔn chibiyɔɔ.
43012025	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nʋ̃ a wʋ nyɛvʋr na bɔr wʋ naa, tɩchɛ 'lɔ na 'laar a wʋ nyɛvʋr a wɛr nyã pɔ, wʋn tara na a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
43012026	Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ sʋ̃ʋ ma tʋ̃, wʋ turo ma, jie jaa ɩn be a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sʋ̃nɔ̃ ma tʋ̃nɔ̃ mɩ na ben be. Ka a n Sãa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a 'lɔ na sʋ̃nɔ̃ ma tʋ̃nɔ̃.
43012027	"Pʋ̃pãanyã, n pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa, tɩ n 'yɛr bo? N 'yɛr ɩka a Sãa wʋ faa ma a sɔ̃ɔ nyãna pɔ bɩɩ? Kai, a sɔ̃ɔ nyãna 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ n wa.
43012028	Sãa, kʋ a fʋ yuor tɩɩr." Be lɛ a kɔkɔr pãa 'yɛr yi saaju, "N dɔ̃ɔ kʋ wʋ a tɩɩr, ɩn lɛ kʋ wʋ naa a tɩɩr go."
43012029	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na ara a be wõ naa na ba 'yɛr, saa lɛ tãna, ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ 'yɛrɛ nɩ wʋ.
43012030	A Yesu 'yɛr ba, "A ba ɩ maa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a kɔkɔr 'yɛr ɛ, tɩ yɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ.
43012031	Pʋ̃pãanyã a sɔ̃ɔ ta naa ka a wɛr nyã 'yɛr na tɔɔr. Pʋ̃pãanyã, ban ir naa wɛr nyã nãa Satan bar.
43012032	Tɩchɛ maa, bala wa 'mɔɔ ma a saaju, ɩn tɔɔn nɩbɛ ba jaa waan a n sɛ̃."
43012033	Wʋ 'yɛr a lɛ na wʋ wiil kũu 'lɔ tɔ wʋn na kpi.
43012034	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala 'yɛr, "Sɩ wõn yi a Nɛɛ pɔ ɩka, a Nɩ-iraa naa 'lɔ na ben be kpo kpo, tɩ ŋmɩnɛ a ɩ a fʋ 'yɛr ɩka ban 'mɔɔn a Nɩsaal Bie a saaju? An lɛ a Nɩsaal Bie 'lɔ?"
43012035	A Yesu pãa 'yɛr ba, "Ber bɩ̃lãa lɛ a chãa na be a yɩ sɛ̃, yɩ chiine a chãa pɔ wʋn chɛnɛ be be ka a libe taa pɔɔ yɩ ɛ. Nɩrɛ na be libe pɔ ba bɔ̃ɔ a jie wʋn chiine ɛ.
43012036	Yɩ sɔɔ de a chãa, yɩn chɛnɛ tara wʋ na yɩ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a chãa bibiir." Yesu na wa 'yɛr a lɛ baar, wʋ yin chen a baa nyɛ wʋ ɛ.
43012037	Yesu gba, wʋn tʋ̃ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ a ba sɛ̃, tɩ baa chɛnɛ sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ.
43012038	Ka a Isaiya 'yɛr ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ. Lɛ wʋn 'yɛr a kõr jaa, "Sɩ Soro an lɛ sɔɔ de a sɩ 'yɛr, an lɛ a Soro mɩ wiil a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ?"
43012039	Ban ba tʋɔrɔ sɔɔrɔ ɛ, bojũu a Isaiya 'yɛr jie ɩ̃sʋɔ,
43012040	"Wʋ jɔ̃ɔn a ba nɩbie bar. Na wʋ pɔɔ a ba tɩɛr bar, baa lɛ nyɛrɛ ɛ. Ba kʋ̃ mɩ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ a par a ba tɩɛr pɔ ɛ, na ba lɩɛb wa a n sɛ̃ ka n sãa ba ɛ."
43012041	Isaiya 'yɛr naa nɩtɔ̃, bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ a Yesu tɩɩr na wʋ 'yɛrɛ a wʋ 'yɛr.
43012042	An sɔɔ be a lɛ tɩ nɩbɛrɛ yɔɔ bamɩne sɔɔn de wʋ. Tɩchɛ a Faraseemɩne dãbɩ̃ɛ jũu baa 'lara 'yɛrɛ ɛ, ka ba taa dii ba bar a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie ɛ.
43012043	Bojũu ba nʋ̃n nɩrɛ pɛɛfʋ gar Nãaŋmɩn pɛɛfʋ.
43012044	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, "Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔɔ de ma a ba ɩ maa tɛɛ lɛ wʋ sɔɔ de ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ sɔɔn de a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma.
43012045	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nyɛ ma mɩ nyɛn a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma.
43012046	N wan a wɛr pɔ nɩtãa chãa, ka nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔɔ de ma kʋ̃ lɛ be libe pɔ ɛ.
43012047	"A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na wõ a n 'yɛr, tɩ na waa tu ɛ, n kʋ̃ tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr ɛ. N ba wa ɩka n wa tɔɔr a wɛr 'yɛr ɛ, tɩ n wa faa wʋ.
43012048	A 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ ben be, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tɔr ma na waa de a n 'yɛr bie ɛ, a 'yɛr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ nɩ wʋ ju ɩn 'yɛr lɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ a 'yɛr a ber baaraa daar.
43012049	N ba 'yɛrɛ n mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ n 'yɛr naa a lɛ a Sãa na tʋ̃ ma 'yɛr ma ɩka n 'yɛr.
43012050	N bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka a wʋ 'yɛr kʋrɔ na nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. Ala lɛ so ka n 'yɛr yɩ a lɛ nɛ a Sãa na 'yɛr."
43013001	A kʋ̃ lɛ kor ɛ, tɩ a Gõl Bar Difʋ ta, Yesu bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a wʋ bɩbir vɩɛ naa ka wʋn yi ka a wɛr nyã pɔ lɩɛb chen a Sãa sɛ̃. Wʋ nʋ̃ naa bala na ɩ a wʋ tʋɔr a wɛr nyã pɔ, wʋ nʋ̃ ban tɩ tãn a wʋ kũu.
43013002	Ba põn a jãanʋɔr bʋ̃diir, ka a ɩ tɩɩ de nie kpɛ Judas na ɩ Simon na yi Isɩkariyot bidaba ka wʋ tɩ gar 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu.
43013003	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a Sãa den bomo a jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ nũu pɔ, an ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ lɛ wʋ yi na wʋ lɛ lɩɛb chiine a wʋ sɛ̃.
43013004	Be lɛ wʋ bar a bʋ̃diir tɩ ir na wʋ yaa a fuu bar tɩ de fɔfɩɛlaa sɛ a sɩɛ pɔ.
43013005	Na wʋ pʋr kʋ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ la'yɛlma pɔ piel pɛɛrɛ a wʋ poturbo gbɛɛ tɩ ma fɩɛl a fɔfɩɛlaa 'lɔ wʋn sɛ a sɩɛ pɔ bar.
43013006	Wʋn wa ta a Simon Pita ka wʋ 'yɛr, "N Soro, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ na pɛɛ a maa gbɛɛ ɔ?"
43013007	A Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "Faa bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ ɩn ɩrɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã ɛ, tɩchɛ fʋn wa bɔ̃ɔn daar kɔ̃ɔ."
43013008	Ka a Pita 'yɛr, "Kai, faa be na wa pɛɛ a n gbɛɛ ɛ." A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Maa ba pɛɛ a fʋ gbɛɛ ɛ, saa lɛ be taa ɛ."
43013009	Ka Simon Pita pãa 'yɛr, "N Soro ala be lɛ, a ta ɩ a gbɛɛ tɛɛ ɛ, pɛɛ a nuur nɩ a ju mɩ."
43013010	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Nɩrɛ na so kʋ̃ɔ baar gbɛɛ tɛɛ lɛ wʋ ma wa pɛɛ, a wʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa yi naa. A yɩn mɩ yi naa an ba ɩ yɩ jaa lɛ ɛ."
43013011	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn a lɔn na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, ala lɛ so ka wʋ 'yɛr ɩka a ba ɩ ba jaa lɛ yi ɛ.
43013012	Wʋn wa pɛɛ a ba jaa gbɛɛ baar, wʋ lɛ den a fuu su tɩ jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a wʋ jie, tɩ sʋʋr ba, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a nɩtɔ̃ ɩn ɩ par ɔ?
43013013	Yɩ ma bʋɔl ma naa Wiwile bɩɩ Soro, yelmɩ̃ɛ yɩ 'yɛr an ɩ a lɛ n ɩ.
43013014	Ala ɩ maa na ɩ a yɩ Soro nɩ a yɩ Wiwile pɛɛn a yɩ gbɛɛ, yɩ mɩ pɛɛrɛ taa gbɛɛ.
43013015	N maal wiil yɩ ɩka yɩ maala a lɛ ɩn ɩ kʋ yɩ.
43013016	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, gbãgbaa ba ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar a wʋ soro ɛ. Tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ mɩ ba ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ wʋ ɛ.
43013017	Pʋ̃pãanyã yɩn bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna, an ɩn sʋ̃ʋfʋ ala ɩ yɩ ɩrɛ yaa naa.
43013018	"Yɩ jaa ba lɛ n 'yɛrɛ ɛ, n bɔ̃ɔ naa a bala ɩn ir. Tɩchɛ lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ na ɩ naa a lɛ an sɛb, 'A 'lɔ ɩn lɔ̃ɔ dire nɩ na lɩɛb ɩ ma bier.'
43013019	"N 'yɛr yɩn a pʋ̃pãanyã tɩchɛ ka a ba ta sɛrɛ ɛ, ala wa ta ka yɩ sɔɔ de ma ɩka Maa lɛ.
43013020	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɔɔ de a 'lɔ ɩn tʋ̃, maa lɛ wʋ sɔɔ de. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na sɔɔ de ma mɩ sɔɔn de a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma."
43013021	Yesu na 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ baar a wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ naa ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na tɩ gar 'yɔ̃ɔ ma."
43013022	Ka a poturbo kaara taa bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bɔ̃ɔ a buor sɔɔ wʋn 'yɛrɛ.
43013023	A Yesu poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ wʋn nʋ̃ na jɛ̃ gbɛb wʋ,
43013024	'lɔ lɛ a Simon Pita 'lɩɩr 'yɛr, "Sʋʋr wʋ kaa, an lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ?"
43013025	Ka a poturo 'lɔ dɩɛl a Yesu tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "N Soro, an lɛ fʋ 'yɛrɛ?"
43013026	A Yesu 'yɛr, "A 'lɔ ɩn na ŋmaa a paanʋ̃ɔ suun a jɩɛr kʋ, 'lɔ lɛ." Wʋ ŋmaa naa a paanʋ̃ɔ suun a jɩɛr de kʋ a Judas na yi Isɩkariyot na ɩ Simon bie.
43013027	Judas na 'wɔb a paanʋ̃ɔ baar ka Satan kpɛ wʋ. Ka Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "A lɛ fʋn bʋɔrɔ ɩka fʋ maal, pɔɔ fɔɔ maal."
43013028	Tɩchɛ a bala na be a bʋ̃diir jie, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba bɔ̃ɔ a par a lɛ Yesu na 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ɛ.
43013029	An ɩ a Judas lɛ tara a ba libie wʋɔ, ka bamɩne tɩɛr ɩka Yesu tɔ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ wʋ ɩka wʋ da bon kɔ̃ɔ waan a ba wa maal a lɔ̃ɔ di jie bɩɩ wʋ kʋ nɔ̃n dẽme bon kɔ̃ɔ.
43013030	A lɛ a Judas na wa de a paanʋ̃ɔ baar wʋ yi naa, tɩ̃sɔɔ mɩ lɛ.
43013031	Wʋn wa yi baar, Yesu 'yɛr naa, "Pʋ̃pãanyã maa Nɩsaal Bie nyɛn tɩɩr ka Nãaŋmɩn mɩ nyɛ tɩɩr tu a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43013032	Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn nyɛn tɩɩr tu a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ naa a Bie tɩɩr, wʋn maal naa lɛ ajienaa.
43013033	"N bibiir, n kʋ̃ lɛ be a yɩ sɛ̃ kor ɛ. Yɩn wa yʋɔrɔ na bʋɔrɔ ma tɩ a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ, lɛ mɩ lɛ n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a pʋ̃pãanyã. A jie 'lɔ ɩn chiine yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wa be ɛ.
43013034	"Bin paalaa lɛ n kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ nʋ̃ taa nɩtãa lɛ ɩn nʋ̃ yɩ. Yɩ mɩ nʋ̃ taa.
43013035	Yɩn wa nʋ̃ taa, nɩbɛ ba jaa na bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka yɩn lɛ ɩ a n poturbo."
43013036	Ka a Simon Pita sʋʋr wʋ, "N Soro, nyɩnɛ fʋ chiine?" A Yesu 'yɛr, "A jie ɩn chiine, fʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tu a pʋ̃pãanyã ɛ, tɩchɛ daar kɔ̃ɔ fʋn tu naa."
43013037	Ka a Pita sʋʋr wʋ, "N Soro, bo lɛ so ka n kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tu fʋ a pʋ̃pãanyã ɛ? Ɩn sɔɔn kpi a fʋ jũu?"
43013038	A Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "Fʋn sɔɔn kpi kʋ ma? Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ ɩka nɔraa kʋ̃ kõ sɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ fʋ chiir gbɛɛ ata ɩka faa bɔ̃ɔ ma ɛ."
43014001	Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a poturbo, "Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a yɩ pʋtɩɛr vavire ɛ, yɩ sɔɔ de Nãaŋmɩn na yɩ mɩ sɔɔ de ma.
43014002	De yɔɔ be na a n Sãa yir, ala ba ta ɩ lɛ ɛ, n kʋ̃ naa 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɛ. N chiine naa na tɩ chɔɔr a jie kʋ yɩ.
43014003	Maa wa chen tɩ chɔɔr a jie baar, ɩn lɩɛb wa de yɩ ka yɩ tɩ be a n sɛ̃, ka yɩ mɩ tɩ be a jie 'lɔ ɩn be.
43014004	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a jie 'lɔ ɩn chiine sɔr."
43014005	Ka Tomasɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "N Soro, sɩn ba bɔ̃ɔ a jie fʋn chiine ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ sɩn ɩrɛ wa bɔ̃ɔ a sɔr?"
43014006	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ a sɔr, a yelmɩ̃ɛ, nɩ a nyɛvʋr. Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ chen a Sãa sɛ̃, na waa tu a n jie ɛ.
43014007	Ala ɩ yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ma naa, yɩn bɔ̃ɔn a Sãa mɩ. An be yi a dɩna yɩ bɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa, na yɩ nyɛ wʋ mɩ."
43014008	Ka Filip 'yɛr, "N Soro, wiil sɩ a Sãa a lɛ na sɛɛ sɩ naa."
43014009	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Filip, a mɔ̃ faa bɔ̃ɔ ma ɔ, a kõr jaa ɩn be a yɩ sɛ̃? Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na nyɛ ma nyɛn a Sãa. Ŋmɩnɛ fʋ 'yɛr ɩka n wiil yɩ a Sãa?
43014010	Faa sɔɔ de ɩka n ben a Sãa 'yɔ̃ɔ ka a Sãa mɩ be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ? A 'yɛrbie ala ɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a ba ɩ maa mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr ɛ, tɩ a Sãa na be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃.
43014011	Yɩ sɔɔ de a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr ɩka n be naa a Sãa 'yɔ̃ɔ ka a Sãa mɩ be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, bɩɩ yɩ sɔɔ de a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala.
43014012	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de ma, wʋn tʋ̃nɔ̃ naa a tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala ɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃. Wʋn tʋ̃n tʋ̃bɛrɛ gar anyãna, bojũu n chiine naa a Sãa sɛ̃.
43014013	Bon jaa yɩn de a yuor sʋɔr, ɩn maal wʋn kʋ yɩ, ka a Sãa nyɛ tɩɩr tu a Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43014014	Yɩ de a n yuor sʋɔr ma bon jaa, ɩn maal wʋ naa.
43014015	"Ala ɩ yɩ nʋ̃ ma naa, yɩn tu naa a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr.
43014016	Ka n sʋɔr a Sãa ka wʋ kʋ yɩ a Sʋ̃nɔ̃ ɩ̃sʋɔ, ka wʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃ jaa kpo kpo.
43014017	A yelmɩ̃ɛ Sɩɛ 'lɔ, a wɛr nɩbɛ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ de wʋ ɛ, bojũu baa nyɛ wʋ ɛ, bɩɩ bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ. Tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ bɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa an ɩ wʋ kpɩɛrɛ naa a yɩ sɛ̃, na wʋn be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43014018	N kʋ̃ bar yɩ nɩtãa kpɩɩr ɛ, ɩn lɩɛb wa a yɩ sɛ̃.
43014019	A chɛn bɩ̃lãa a wɛr nɩbɛ kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ ma go ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ na nyɛ ma naa. Bojũu ɩn tara na nyɛvʋr ka yɩn mɩ na a nyɛvʋr.
43014020	A bɩbir 'lɔ wa vɩɛ, yɩn bɔ̃ɔ ɩka n be naa a n Sãa 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka yɩ mɩ be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka n mɩ be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43014021	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na de a n 'yɛr na wʋ turo, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nʋ̃ ma. 'Lɔ jaa mɩ na nʋ̃ ma, a n Sãa mɩ na nʋ̃ wʋ naa, ka maa mɩ nʋ̃ a nɩnyɩnɛ, naa wiil wʋ a n mɩ̃ɛ."
43014022	Be lɛ ka a Judas, a ba ɩ a Judas 'lɔ na yi a Isɩkariyot ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ 'yɛr, "Tɩchɛ, n Soro bo lɛ so ka fʋ wiil a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ sɩ, tɩ na faa wile a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋrɔ a wɛr nɩbɛ ɛ."
43014023	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa nʋ̃ ma naa, wʋn turo naa a n wiilfʋ. A n Sãa na nʋ̃ wʋ naa, ka sɩ wa be a wʋ sɛ̃.
43014024	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba nʋ̃ ma ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tu a n wiilfʋ ɛ. A 'yɛrbie anyãna yɩn wõ ba ɩ maa mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr ɛ, a yin a Sãa na tʋ̃ ma sɛ̃.
43014025	"A anyãna a jaa lɛ n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ, ɩn chɛnɛ be a yɩ sɛ̃.
43014026	Tɩchɛ a Sʋ̃nɔ̃ 'lɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ, 'lɔ lɛ a Sãa na tʋ̃n a n yuor. Wʋn wiil yɩ naa a yele a jaa, na wʋ mɩ jɛɔ yɩ ala a jaa ɩn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr yɩ.
43014027	Nyã'maar pɔ lɛ n bar yɩ, a maa mɩ̃ɛ nyã'maar lɛ n bar kʋ yɩ. N ba kʋ yɩ nɩtãa lɛ a wɛr nɩbɛ na ma kʋ ɛ. Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka yɩ tɩɛr vavire ɛ, ka yɩ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
