43014028	"Yɩ wõn a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr ɩka n chiine naa tɩ ɩn lɩɛb wa a yɩ sɛ̃. Ala ɩ yɩ ta nʋ̃ ma naa, yɩ pʋɔ naa pɛl naa ɩn chiine a Sãa sɛ̃ an ɩ a n Sãa lɛ bɛrma gar ma.
43014029	N den nie 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, tɩchɛ ka a na wa ɩ, ala wa ɩ, yɩn sɔɔn de.
43014030	Maa nɩ yɩn kʋ̃ lɛ 'yɛr kor ɛ, bojũu a wɛr nyã nãa Satan waara naa, tɩ waa tara kpɛ̃ɔ a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
43014031	Tɩchɛ a wɛr nɩbɛ na bɔ̃ɔn ɩka n nʋ̃ naa n Sãa naa maal a lɛ nɛ a n Sãa na 'yɔ̃ɔ ma. Yɩ ir a sɩ chen."
43015001	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ ɩ a tɩwɔ̃n sʋ̃ ka a n Sãa mɩ ɩ a tɩkaara.
43015002	Wʋ ma ŋman a wilsɩ ala na be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ tɩ ba wɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ. A wilsɩ ala mɩ na wɔ̃nɔ̃, wʋ ma chɔɔr 'mɛl bar ka a wɔ̃ yɔɔ.
43015003	Yɩn 'lɔ, a 'yɛr ɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ chɔɔr yɩ naa.
43015004	Yɩ mar a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka n mɩ mar a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ. Wile jaa kʋ̃ wɔ̃ wɔ̃mɔ̃ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, ka waa mar a tɩwɔ̃naa 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ. Yɩn mɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wɔ̃mɔ̃ wɔ̃ ɛ. Yɩn mɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wɔ̃mɔ̃ wɔ̃ ɛ, ka yaa mar a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
43015005	"Maa lɛ ɩ a tɩɛ, yɩn mɩ lɛ a wilsɩ, ala ɩ nɩrɛ be naa a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ka n mɩ be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, wʋn wɔ̃n wɔ̃mɔ̃ yɔɔ. Maa ba be a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ, yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bon jaa ɩ ɛ.
43015006	Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, wʋ nyɛntãan a wile ban lɔb bar ka wʋ ko. Ba ma wob a wilbie anyãna lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ bũu pɔ ka a di.
43015007	Ala ɩ yɩ be naa a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a n 'yɛr be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, yɩ sʋɔr bon jaa yɩn bʋɔrɔ, yɩn nyɛ naa.
43015008	A nyã lɛ ɩ a n Sãa tɩɩr yɩn wa wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃mɔ̃ yɔɔ, a mɩ nɩ wiil naa ɩka yɩ ɩ naa n poturbo.
43015009	"Lɛ a Sãa na nʋ̃ ma, lɛ mɩ lɛ n nʋ̃ yɩ. Yɩ ara a n nʋ̃fʋ pɔ.
43015010	Ala ɩ yɩ tu naa a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr, yɩn be naa a n nʋ̃fʋ pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ ɩn tu a n Sãa 'yɛr naa be a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ pɔ.
43015011	A anyãna lɛ n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ka n pʋpɛl be a yɩ sɛ̃, ka a yɩ chɩlfʋ mɩ sɛɛ.
43015012	A n 'yɛr ɩn kʋrɔ yɩ nɩ nyã. Yɩ nʋ̃ taa nɩtãa lɛ ɩn nʋ̃ yɩ.
43015013	A nʋ̃fʋ 'lɔ na gar a nʋ̃fʋ a jaa lɛ nɩrɛ na sɔɔ kpi kʋ a wʋ barmɩne.
43015014	Yɩn lɛ ɩ a n barmɩne ala ɩ yɩ ɩrɛ naa a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr.
43015015	N ba lɛ bʋɔlɔ yɩ gbãgbaar go ɛ, bojũu tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ba bɔ̃ɔ lɛ a wʋ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na ɩrɛ ɛ. N bʋɔlɔ yɩ naa n barmɩne, bojũu n 'yɛr yɩn a lɛ jaa ɩn wõ yi a n Sãa sɛ̃.
43015016	Yɩn baa ir ma ɛ, tɩchɛ maa lɛ ir yɩ ɩka yɩ tɩ wɔ̃ wɔ̃mɔ̃, a wɔ̃mɔ̃ ala na kʋ̃ sɔ̃ɔ ɛ. A Sãa na pãa kʋ yɩ naa bon jaa yɩn sʋɔr a n yuor pɔ.
43015017	A nyãna lɛ n 'yɛr ɩka, yɩ nʋ̃ taa.
43015018	"Ala wa ɩ a wɛr nɩbɛ 'laar yɩ naa, yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka ba dɔ̃ɔ de nie 'laar ma.
43015019	Ala ɩ yɩ ta ɩ naa a wɛr nɩbɛ, a wɛr nɩbɛ naa nʋ̃ yɩ naa nɩtãa a wʋ bon. Yaa ɩ a wɛr nyã tʋɔr ɛ. Tɩchɛ an ɩ n oo yɩn ir a wɛr nɩbɛ pɔ, ala lɛ so a ba 'laar yɩ.
43015020	Yɩ tɩɛr tɔ a 'yɛr 'lɔ ɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ. Gbãgbaa ba ɩ kpɛ̃ɛ gar a wʋ soro ɛ. Ala ɩ ba ge ma naa, ba mɩ na ge yɩ naa. Ala ɩ ba tu naa a n wiilfʋ, ba mɩ a n tu naa a yɩ wiilfʋ mɩ.
43015021	Ban maal yɩ naa a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ a n yuor jũu, bojũu baa bɔ̃ɔ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma ɛ.
43015022	Ala ɩ n ba ta wa 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ ba ɛ, ba kʋ̃ naa tara yeldɛɛr ɛ, pʋ̃pãanyã baa tara a ba yeldɛɛr lɩɛb tunfʋ jie ɛ.
43015023	A 'lɔ na 'laar ma mɩ 'laara a n Sãa mɩ.
43015024	Maa ta ba tʋ̃tʋ̃mɔ̃ na ba sɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ jaa na ba ɩ ɛ, ba kʋ̃ naa tara yeldɛɛr ɛ. Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã ba nyɛn a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɩn tʋ̃, tɩ chɛnɛ 'laar ma nɩ a n Sãa.
43015025	Tɩchɛ a anyã ɩ naa ka a ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ a lɛ an sɛb a Nɛɛ pɔ, 'Ba 'laar man pɔrɔ.'
43015026	"A Sʋ̃nɔ̃ na wa na, a 'lɔ na yi a Sãa sɛ̃. A yelmɩ̃ɛ Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋ yin a Sãa sɛ̃, wʋn 'yɛr yɩ naa a n 'yɛr.
43015027	Yɩ mɩ na 'yɛr naa a n 'yɛr bojũu yɩ ben a n sɛ̃ a pielfʋ jaa."
43016001	A Yesu 'yɛr, "A anyãna a jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, ka yɩ taa bar yi a sɔɔfʋ pɔ ɛ.
43016002	Ban dii yɩn bar a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie. Bɩbir kɔ̃ɔ na vɩɛ naa, ka ba kʋ yɩ tɩ tɩɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ ba tʋ̃.
43016003	Ban ɩ naa anyãna, bojũu baa bɔ̃ɔ a Sãa ɛ, bɩɩ a maa ɛ.
43016004	N 'yɛrɛ yɩ naa anyãna ka a bɩbir wa vɩɛ yɩn tɩɛr tɔ, ɩka n dɔ̃ɔ kpãa yɩ. N ba dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɛ, bojũu n be naa a yɩ sɛ̃.
43016005	"Pʋ̃pãanyã n chiine naa a 'lɔ na tʋ̃ ma sɛ̃, tɩchɛ a ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba sʋʋr ma a jie ɩn chiine ɛ.
43016006	A anyãna ɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ jũu lɛ a yɩ pʋʋr sɔ̃ɔ ɔ?
43016007	Tɩchɛ yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a yɩ jũu a sɛɛ naa ɩka n chen. Maa ba chen ɛ, a Sʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋ̃ wa a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ maa chen ɩn tʋ̃ wʋn ka wʋ wa a yɩ sɛ̃.
43016008	'Lɔ wa wa, wʋn wiil a wɛr nɩbɛ a ba bɔ̃ɔ ɩka ba bɔr naa, lɛ a yeldɛɛr nɩ yeltorsɩ na be, nɩ lɛ wʋn na tɔɔr a ba 'yɛr.
43016009	Wʋn vɛ̃ naa a ba bɔ̃ɔ a ba yeldɛɛr ban ba sɔɔ de ma ɛ.
43016010	Ba bɔr naa nɩ a yeltorsɩ, bojũu n chiine naa a Sãa sɛ̃, yɩ kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ ma go ɛ.
43016011	Ba mɩ bɔr naa nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ yele, bojũu a wɛr nyã nãa Satan 'yɛr tɔɔr naa.
43016012	"N chɛnɛ na tara 'yɛr yɔɔ nɩ taa 'yɛr yɩ tɩchɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ.
43016013	Tɩchɛ a yelmɩ̃ɛ Sɩɛ 'lɔ wa wa, wʋn wiil yɩ naa a yelmɩ̃ɛ wʋ jaa par. Wʋ kʋ̃ 'yɛr a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ wʋn 'yɛr naa a lɛ tɛɛ wʋn wõ, na wʋ lɛ 'yɛr yɩ a ala na wa.
43016014	Wʋn waan na tɩɩr wa kʋ ma, na wʋ vɛ̃ ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a ala na ɩ a n bon.
43016015	Ala a jaa a Sãa na so ɩ naa a n bon. Ala lɛ so ka n 'yɛr ɩka a Sɩɛ na vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a ala na ɩ a n bon.
43016016	"A chɛn bɩ̃lãa yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ ma go ɛ, ka a pãa lɛ ɩ bɩ̃lãa ka yɩ nyɛ ma go."
43016017	Ka a poturbo bamɩne sʋrɔ taa, "A par nɩ bo wʋn 'yɛr ɛ ɩka, 'A chɛn bɩ̃lãa yɩ kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ ma go ɛ, ka a pãa lɛ ɩ bɩ̃lãa ka yɩ lɛ nyɛ wʋ go, nɩ wʋn lɛ 'yɛr ɩka, n chiine naa a Sãa sɛ̃?' "
43016018	Ba chɛnɛ na sʋrɔ taa, "A chɛn bɩ̃lãa par nɩ bo? 'Sãa bɔ̃ɔ a par a lɛ,' wʋn 'yɛrɛ ɛ."
43016019	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn naa ban bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba sʋʋr wʋ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ sʋrɔ nɩ taa a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr ɩka, 'A chɛn bɩ̃lãa yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ ma go ɛ, ka a lɛ ɩ bɩ̃lãa ka yɩ nyɛ ma go'?
43016020	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩn kõnõ na ka yɩ pʋʋr sɔ̃ɔ, tɩchɛ ka a wɛr nɩbɛ chɩlɛ. Yɩ pʋʋr na sɔ̃ɔ naa, tɩchɛ ka a yɩ pʋsɔ̃ɔ na lɩɛb pʋpɛl.
43016021	Pɔɔ wa dɔɔrɔ ɩ̃gãn ma chɩrɛ wʋ naa ka a ɔɔrɔ wʋ bojũu a wʋ dɔɔfʋ bɩbir vɩɛ naa. Tɩchɛ 'lɔ wʋ dɔɔ baar, wʋ ma ĩin naa a wʋ dɔɔyɛ bojũu wʋ dɔɔn nɩrɛ a wɛr pɔ.
43016022	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ a yɩn mɩ, yɩ pʋʋr na sɔ̃ɔ naa a pʋ̃pãanyã, tɩchɛ ɩn lɛ wa nyɛ yɩn go ka yɩ pʋʋl pɛl, ka a nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ faa wʋ ɛ.
43016023	A bɩbir 'lɔ wa vɩɛ, yɩ kʋ̃ lɛ sʋʋr ma bon go ɛ. Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a n Sãa na kʋ yɩn bon jaa yɩn sʋɔr a n yuor pɔ.
43016024	An wa ta a pʋ̃pãanyã, yaa de a n yuor sʋɔr bon gba ɛ. Yɩ sʋɔr, yɩn nyɛ naa, ka yɩ pʋpɛl na sɛɛ.
43016025	"Sʋkpar lɛ n lɔɔrɔ 'yɛrɛ nɩ yɩ a anyãna, a bɩbir wa vɩɛ, n kʋ̃ lɛ lɔb sʋkpar go ɛ, tɩchɛ ɩn 'yɛr yɩ naa a n Sãa 'yɛr chãa pɔ.
43016026	A bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, yɩn sʋɔr naa nɩ a n yuor. N ba 'yɛrɛ ɩka maa lɛ na sʋɔr a Sãa kʋ yɩ ɛ.
43016027	An ɩ a Sãa nʋ̃ yɩ naa bojũu yɩ nʋ̃ ma naa na yɩ sɔɔ de ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ lɛ n yi.
43016028	A Sãa sɛ̃ lɛ n yi wa ka a wɛr pɔ, pʋ̃pãanyã n lɛ bara naa a wɛr tɩ lɩɛb chiine a Sãa sɛ̃."
43016029	Ka a Yesu poturbo pãa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Pʋ̃pãanyã fʋ pãa 'yɛr ka a chaar faa lɛ lɔɔrɔ sʋkpar go ɛ.
43016030	Pʋ̃pãanyã sɩ nyɛn ɩka fʋ bɔ̃ɔn yele a jaa, na faa lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ sʋʋr fʋ sʋʋrfʋsɩ ɛ. Ala lɛ so ka sɩ sɔɔ de ɩka Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ lɛ fʋ yi."
43016031	Ka a Yesu sʋʋr ba, "Yɩ pãa sɔɔn de a pʋ̃pãanyã ɔ?
43016032	Tɩchɛ bɩbir kɔ̃ɔ na wa vɩɛ naa, wʋ ben ta, ka yɩ jaa na yɛ̃yɛl ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kul a wʋ yir tɩ chɛ ma bar a n yõ. Tɩ n ba ɩ a n yõ ɛ, a n Sãa be naa n sɛ̃.
43016033	"N 'yɛr yɩ naa anyãna ka yɩ na tara nyã'maar an ɩ yɩ ben a n 'yɔ̃ɔ. A wɛr nyã pɔ yɩn din dɔɔyɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ nyɔɔ nyãa, bojũu n tʋ̃ɔn a wɛr."
43017001	A Yesu na wa 'yɛr a anyãna baar, wʋ kãan saaju tɩ 'yɛr, "N Sãa, a bɩbir vɩɛ naa, kʋ a fʋ Bie a tɩɩr ka a fʋ Bie mɩ kʋ fʋ a tɩɩr.
43017002	Bojũu, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ kʋ wʋ sɔr ka wʋ tʋ̃ɔ a nɩbɛ ba jaa na wʋ kʋ ba a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, a bala ba jaa fʋn de kʋ wʋ.
43017003	A nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ nɩ nyã, ka ban bɔ̃ɔ a fʋ̃ʋ Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ, na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, nɩ a Yesu 'lɔ fʋn tʋ̃.
43017004	N waan na tɩɩr wa kʋ fʋ a ka a wɛr pɔ, naa baar a tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala fʋn kʋ ma ɩka n tʋ̃.
43017005	Pʋ̃pãanyã, n Sãa kʋ ma a tɩɩr a fʋ niem, a tɩɩr 'lɔ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ tara tɩchɛ na fʋ wa maal a wɛr.
43017006	"N wiil fʋn kʋ a bala fʋn de kʋ ma ka a wɛr pɔ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ so ba tɩ na fʋ wa de ba kʋ ma, ba tu naa a fʋ 'yɛr.
43017007	Pʋ̃pãanyã ba bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka bon jaa ɩn tara yin a fʋ sɛ̃.
43017008	Bojũu, a 'yɛr ala fʋn kʋ ma, n 'yɛr kʋ ba, ka ba sɔɔ de. Ba bɔ̃ɔn yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa ɩka fʋ̃ʋ sɛ̃ lɛ n yi naa wa, na ba sɔɔ de ɩka fʋ̃ʋ lɛ tʋ̃ ma.
43017009	Bala 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ n sʋɔrɔ fʋ, n ba sʋɔrɔ fʋ kʋrɔ a wɛr nɩbɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala fʋn kʋ ma an ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ so ba.
43017010	Bon jaa ɩn tara ɩ naa a fʋ sofʋ, ka bon jaa fʋn mɩ na tara ɩ a n sofʋ. N nyɛn tɩɩr yi a ba jie.
43017011	Maa kʋ̃ lɛ be ka a wɛr pɔ go ɛ, tɩchɛ bala 'lɔ chɛnɛ na be ka a wɛr pɔ, n waara a fʋ sɛ̃. Sãa sʋ̃, gu ba nɩ a fʋ yuor kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ pɔ, a yuor 'lɔ fʋn kʋ ma ka ban ɩ bʋ̃'yen, nɩtãa lɛ maa nɩ fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ bʋ̃'yen.
43017012	Ɩn be a ba sɛ̃, n gu ban naa kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ fʋn kʋ ma. Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba bɔr ɛ, ala ba ɩ a 'lɔ tɛɛ an sɛɛ ɩka wʋ bɔr ka a lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43017013	"N waara naa a fʋ sɛ̃ a pʋ̃pãanyã, tɩchɛ ɩn chɛnɛ be ka a wɛr pɔ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ a anyãna ka ban tara a n pʋpɛl wʋ jaa.
43017014	N kʋ ban a fʋ 'yɛr, ala lɛ so ka a wɛr nɩbɛ 'laar ba, baa lɛ chɛnɛ pʋɔ ba go ɛ, nɩtãa maa na ba pʋɔ ba ɛ.
43017015	N ba sʋɔrɔ fʋ ɩka fʋ ir ba yin ka a wɛr pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ fʋ guro ba a dɛɛr sʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43017016	Baa lɛ pʋɔ a wɛr nɩbɛ pɔ ɛ, nɩtãa n mɩ na ba pʋɔ ba ɛ.
43017017	Oo ba nɩ a fʋ yelmɩ̃ɛ, a fʋ 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43017018	Nɩtãa lɛ fʋn tʋ̃ ma a wɛr nɩbɛ sɛ̃, lɛ lɛ n mɩ tʋ̃ ba a wɛr nɩbɛ sɛ̃.
43017019	A ba 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ n oo a n mɩ̃ɛ kʋ fʋ, ka ba mɩ na oo a ba mɩ̃ɛ sɩrɛ jaa kʋ fʋ.
43017020	"A ba ɩ bala tɛɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ n sʋɔrfʋ ɛ, n mɩ sʋɔrɔ na kʋrɔ a bala na wa sɔɔ de ma tu a ba 'yɔ̃ɔ.
43017021	N sʋɔrɔ fʋ naa ɩka fʋ vɛ̃ ka ba jaa ɩ bʋ̃'yen. N Sãa, nɩtãa lɛ fʋn be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka n mɩ be a fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ. Ba mɩ be a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ ka a wɛr nɩbɛ na sɔɔ de ɩka fʋ̃ʋ lɛ tʋ̃ ma.
43017022	N kʋ ban a tɩɩr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ nɩ wʋ ju fʋn kʋ ma, ka ba na ɩ bʋ̃'yen nɩtãa maa nɩ fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ bʋ̃'yen.
43017023	N ben a ba 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka fʋ mɩ be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ. Ka ba jaa mɩ na 'mataa ɩ bʋ̃'yen ka a wɛr nɩbɛ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka fʋ̃ʋ lɛ tʋ̃ ma na fʋ nʋ̃ ba gba nɩtãa a lɛ fʋn nʋ̃ ma.
43017024	"N Sãa, n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka a bala fʋn kʋ ma, ba mɩ be a jie 'lɔ ɩn na be, na ba nyɛ a n tɩɩr. A tɩɩr 'lɔ fʋn de nie kʋ ma, bojũu fʋ nʋ̃ ma naa tɩ na fʋ wa maal a wɛr.
43017025	"N Sãa, a fʋ yele tor naa, tɩ a wɛr nɩbɛ ba bɔ̃ɔ fʋ ɛ, maa bɔ̃ɔ fʋ naa, ka a n poturbo mɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka fʋ̃ʋ lɛ tʋ̃ ma.
43017026	N vɛ̃n ka ba bɔ̃ɔ fʋ, ɩn chɛnɛ na maal ba ka ba bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ fʋ pʋɔrɔ ka a nʋ̃fʋ 'lɔ fʋn nʋ̃ ma na be a ba 'yɔ̃ɔ ka n mɩ be a ba 'yɔ̃ɔ."
43018001	Yesu na sʋɔr a Sãa a nɩtɔ̃ baar, 'lɔ naa poturbo gɔ̃ɔ naa a Kidɩrɔn kʋla gɔ̃ɔn. 'Lɔ nɩ a wʋ poturbo chen a jie a kãa tɩɩr na be.
43018002	Judas na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ mɩ bɔ̃ɔn a jie nyã, bojũu Yesu naa wʋ poturbo ba gala a be lɔ̃ɔfʋ ɛ.
43018003	Be lɛ Judas tara a Worom sojasɩ, nɩ a puorfʋ die gugurbo bala a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Faraseemɩne na tʋ̃ chiin a jie 'lɔ. Ba tara na bũusɩ, fɩ̃tɩnsɩ nɩ jɛɛr bomo.
43018004	Yesu na bɔ̃ɔ lɛ na waara a wʋ sɛ̃, wʋ tuor sʋʋr ba, "An yɩ bʋɔrɔ?"
43018005	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Yesu na yi Najaretɩ lɛ sɩ bʋɔrɔ." Ka a Yesu 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ." Ka a Judas 'lɔ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ lɔ̃ɔn ba ara.
43018006	Yesu na wa 'yɛr ɩka, "Maa lɛ." Ba lɩɛb puor lo lo tẽe.
43018007	Wʋ lɛ sʋʋr ban go, "An lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ?" A ba 'yɛr, "Yesu na yi Najaretɩ."
43018008	A Yesu 'yɛr, "N ba 'yɛr yɩ ɩka 'Maa lɛ.' Ala ɩ maa lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ, yɩ ɩ ka a nɩbɛ banyã chiine."
43018009	Yesu 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ ka a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka, "A bala fʋn kʋ ma, n ba vɛ̃ ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa bɔr ɛ."
43018010	Be lɛ a Simon Pita na tara sʋɔ na wʋ vʋ̃ɔ chɛn a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ gbãgbaa nũsʋ̃ɔ toor ŋmaa. A gbãgbaa yuor din Malkusɩ.
43018011	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ a Pita, "Su a sʋɔ a sʋkpa pɔ, n ta nyũn a dɔɔyɛ ŋmele 'lɔ a Sãa na kʋ ma bɩɩ?"
43018012	Ka a sojasɩ nɩ a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'matãan a gugurbo bala ban tʋ̃, nyɔɔ a Yesu na ba lũ.
43018013	Ba den nie tara wʋ chiin Anasɩ sɛ̃, wʋ ɩ naa a Kayafasɩ dɩ̃ɛ na wʋ mɩ ɩ bɔɔrlo nãa a yuon 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
43018014	A Kayafasɩ nyãna lɛ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ ɩka a ɩn sʋ̃, ka nɩbʋ̃'yen na kpi kʋ a nɩbɛ.
43018015	Simon Pita nɩ a poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ turo naa a Yesu, bojũu a poturo nyã bɔ̃ɔn a bɔɔrlo nãa ala lɛ so ka wʋ tu a Yesu kpɛ a bɔɔrlo nãa bɛchaar pɔ.
43018016	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita 'lɔ ara a yõo dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ. A poturo nyã a bɔɔrlo nãa na bɔ̃ɔ, yin wa 'yɛr a pɔɔbile 'lɔ na kaara a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ tɩ tara a Pita kpɛ̃n.
43018017	Ka a pɔɔbile 'lɔ na kaara a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ, sʋʋr a Pita, "A fʋ̃ʋ, faa mɩ ɩ a daba nyã poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ?" Ka a Pita 'yɛr, "N ba ɩ a wʋ poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ."
43018018	Ɔɔr kʋrɔ naa ka a gbãgbaar nɩ a gugurbo bala gbɔɔ saalaa bũu ara uoro ka a Pita mɩ tɩ ara uoro.
43018019	A bɔɔrlo nãa sʋʋr naa a Yesu, ba boo lɛ ɩ a wʋ poturbo nɩ bo lɛ wʋ ma wile?
43018020	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Chãa pɔ lɛ n ma 'yɛrɛ a n 'yɛr kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ. N ma wile ba naa a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie nɩ a ba Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ jiir, be lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ ba jaa ma lɔ̃ɔ. N ba sɔɔl 'yɛr 'yɛr jaa ɛ.
43018021	Bo lɛ so ka fʋ sʋrɔ ma a lɛ? Sʋʋr a bala na wõ a n 'yɛr, ba bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr."
43018022	Yesu na 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ ka a guguro ɩ̃sʋɔ na ara gbʋr wʋ 'ma wʋ tɩ 'yɛr, "Lɛ lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka fʋ 'yɛr kʋ a bɔɔrlo nãa ɔ?"
43018023	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr n bɔr naa, wiil a n bɔrfʋ jie. Tɩchɛ ala ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n mɩ 'yɛr, bo 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ 'ma ma?"
43018024	Wʋ chɛnɛ na lũ tɩchɛ ka a Anasɩ vɛ̃ a ba tara wʋ chiin a bɔɔrlo nãa Kayafasɩ sɛ̃.
43018025	A Simon Pita na chɛnɛ ara uoro a bũu, ba sʋʋr wʋ naa, "A fʋ̃ʋ, fʋ ɩ naa a daba nyã poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ɔ?" Ka Pita chiir 'yɛr, "N ba ɩ a wʋ poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ."
43018026	A bɔɔrlo nãa gbãgbaa ɩ̃sʋɔ, wʋ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ toor lɛ a 'lɔ a Pita na dɔ̃ɔ chɛ ŋmaa 'yɛr, "A ba ɩ n nyɛ fʋ naa fʋn be a wʋ sɛ̃ a kãa tɩɩr jie 'lɔ ɛ?"
43018027	Ka a Pita lɛ chiir, ka a nɔraa mɩ tɔ̃ɔ kõ ajienaa.
43018028	Be lɛ ba tara a Yesu yin a Kayafasɩ yir bibio pipi na ba chiin a Worom nɩkpɛ̃ɛ yir. A Juu nɩbɛ mɩ̃ɛ ba kpɛ be ɛ, bojũu baa bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba sɔ̃ɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ na ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ di a Gõl Bar Difʋ ɛ.
43018029	Lɛ lɛ a Pilate yi a yõo tɩ sʋʋr ba, "Bo yelbier yɩ ɩka a daba nyã ɩ naa?"
43018030	Ka ba 'yɛr, "'Lɔ ba ta maal yelbier ɛ, sɩ kʋ̃ naa tara wʋ waan a fʋ sɛ̃ ɛ."
43018031	Ka Pilate 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ, yɩ de wʋ tɩ tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr, a lɛ a yɩn mɩ̃ɛ nɛɛ na 'yɛr bin." Tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ 'yɛr, "Saa tara sɔr na kʋ nɩrɛ ɛ."
43018032	A ɩn a lɛ a Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr wiil a kũu 'lɔ tɔ wʋn na kpi.
43018033	Pilate lɩɛb kpɛ tɩ bʋɔl a Yesu sʋʋr, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa bɩɩ?"
43018034	A Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ tɩɛr a lɛ bɩɩ nɩbɛ lɛ 'yɛr a n 'yɛr kʋ fʋ?"
43018035	Ka a Pilate 'yɛr, "Fʋ tɩɛr ɩka n ɩn Juu nɩrɛ bɩɩ? A fʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ nɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ baa nyɔɔ fʋ waan a n sɛ̃, bo fʋ̃ʋ ɩ?"
43018036	A Yesu 'yɛr, "A n nãalʋ̃ʋ ba yi ka a wɛr pɔ ɛ, ala ɩ a wɛr pɔ lɛ wʋ dɔ̃ɔ yi, a n poturbo naa jɛb faa ma ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ ta nyɔɔ ma ɛ. Tɩchɛ a n nãalʋ̃ʋ ba yi a ka ɛ."
43018037	Ka a Pilate pãa sʋʋr wʋ, "Ka ala ɩ a lɛ, nãa lɛ fʋ ɩ wɛ?" Ka Yesu 'yɛr, "Fʋ 'yɛr vɩla fʋn 'yɛr ɩka nãa lɛ n ɩ, ala 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ ba dɔɔ ma ka n wa ka a wɛr pɔ, naa wa 'yɛr a yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ chɛlɛ naa lɛ ɩn 'yɛrɛ."
43018038	Ka Pilate sʋʋr wʋ, "Bo lɛ ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ?" Wʋn sʋʋr a nɩtɔ̃ baar, wʋ yin a yõo a Juu nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "N ba nyɛ yelsɔ̃ɔnaa jaa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
43018039	Tɩchɛ a yɩ binfʋ lɛ ɩka n ma ir nɩrɛ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ kʋ yɩ a Gõl Bar Difʋ daar. Yɩ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n yuo a yɩ nãa kʋ yɩ bɩɩ?"
43018040	A ba tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Kai, saa bʋɔrɔ wʋ ɛ, Barabasɩ lɛ sɩ bʋɔrɔ." Tɩchɛ a Barabasɩ mɩ ɩn nɩkʋrɔ.
43019001	Pilate vɛ̃ naa ka ba nyɔɔ a Yesu chiin tɩ fɔb.
43019002	Ka a sojasɩ de gʋʋr wob jupil su a Yesu, tɩ mɩ de fuu jɩ̃ ile ile na ba su wʋ.
43019003	Tɩ pãa ma tɔɔ ta a wʋ sɛ̃ 'yɛrɛ, "Sɩ puor fʋ naa Juu nɩbɛ nãa," tɩ ma 'ma 'ma wʋ.
43019004	Pilate lɛ yin wa a Juu nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃ go wa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ nyɛ, ɩn vɛ̃n ka ba yi waan wʋ, ka yɩn mɩ̃ɛ nyɛ ɩka, n ba nyɛ yelbier jaa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ."
43019005	Ban wa yin a Yesu, wʋ sun a gʋʋr jupil nɩ a fuu jɩ̃ ile ile 'lɔ, ka a Pilate 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ nyɛ a daba."
43019006	A bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a puorfʋ yir gugurbo, ban wa nyɛ a Yesu, ka ba tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Kpa wʋ a daa ju. Kpa wʋ a daa ju." Tɩchɛ ka a Pilate 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn, yɩ de wʋ tɩ kpa wʋ a daa ju, maa 'lɔ n ba nyɛ yelbier jaa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ."
43019007	Tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ 'yɛr, "Sɩ tara na nɛɛ, sɩn 'yɛr, ka a nɛɛ 'lɔ ɩka wʋ sɛɛn kũu, bojũu wʋ bʋɔlɔ naa wʋ mɩ̃ɛ Nãaŋmɩn Bie."
43019008	Pilate na wõ a nɩtɔ̃ ka dãbɩ̃ɛ gba kpɛ wʋ.
43019009	Ka wʋ lɩɛb kpɛ na wʋ tɩ sʋʋr a Yesu, "Nyɩnɛ fʋ yi?" Tɩchɛ Yesu ba haa nɛɛ sɔɔ wʋ ɛ.
43019010	A Pilate sʋʋr wʋ, "Faa haar ma nɛɛ ɛ? Faa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka n tara na sɔr na vɛ̃ ka ba kʋ fʋ, naa lɛ tara sɔr na faar fʋ bar ɛ?"
43019011	Be lɛ a Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "Faa tara kpɛ̃ɔ bɩ̃lãa jaa a n jie ɛ, ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn ba de yin saaju kʋ fʋ ɛ. A lɛ jũu nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nyɔɔ ma wa kʋ fʋ, wʋ lon yeldɛɛr pɔ gar fʋ."
43019012	An yi a be chiine, ka Pilate pãa mʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ faar a Yesu, tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Fʋ̃ʋ vɛ̃ ka a daba nyã chen, faa ɩ a Siisa baraa go ɛ. Nɩrɛ jaa na ɩka nãa lɛ wʋ ɩ, wʋ jɛɛrɛ nɩ naa a Siisa."
43019013	Pilate na wõ a nɩtɔ̃, wʋ yin naa Yesu tɩ jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ dakɔɔ ju, a jie ban bʋɔlɔ Kʋsɩpãn. Ka a Juu nɩbɛrɛ mɩ bʋɔlɔ a jie Gabata.
43019014	A Gõl Bar Difʋ bɩ̃nsɩ daar mɔ̃tɔ̃tuo sɔ̃ɔ, Pilate 'yɛr kʋ a Juu nɩbɛrɛ, "Yɩ nyɛ a yɩ nãa."
43019015	Tɩchɛ ka ba tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Kʋ wʋ. Kʋ wʋ. Kpa wʋ yɔɔl a daa ju." Ka a Pilate sʋʋr ba, "N kpa a yɩ nãa?" A ba 'yɛrɛ, "Saa tara nãa jaa ka nãa Siisa ba lɛ ɛ."
43019016	Ka Pilate vɛ̃ a ba nyɔɔ a Yesu chiin na tɩ kpa ka a sojasɩ tara wʋ.
43019017	Yesu yin tuo a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ daa chiin a jie 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Julaa Jie. Tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ mɩ bʋɔlɔ a jie, Gɔlgɔta.
43019018	Be lɛ ba kpa wʋ 'matãan nɩbɛ ayi, ka bala be a lõbobo tɩchɛ ka a Yesu be a sãlsɔɔ.
43019019	Pilate sɛb sɛbie 'mar a daa ju ɩka, YESU NA YI NAJARETƖ, A JUU NƖBƐ NÃA.
43019020	Kɔkɔɛ ata lɛ wʋ sɛb, a Juu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr, Worom nɩbɛ kɔkɔr nɩ a Greek dẽme kɔkɔr. Ka a Juu nɩbɛ yɔɔ kar a sɛbie bojũu a jie ban kpa wʋ ba jãan a yir ɛ.
43019021	Ka a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ 'yɛr kʋ a Pilate, "Ta sɛb ɩka a Juu nɩbɛ nãa ɛ, fʋn taa sɛb ɩka a daba nyã 'yɛr ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nãa."
43019022	Ka a Pilate 'yɛr, "A lɛ ɩn sɛb n sɛb baar."
43019023	A sojasɩ na wa kpa a Yesu baar, ba põn a wʋ fuusɩ jiir anaar ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa 'mɔɔ wʋ bon. A wa chɛn a fuu wõo 'lɔ na ba tara nɛɛ ɛ, bʋ̃bʋ̃'yen lɛ ba wob yin a saaju tɩ baar a gbɛɛ pɔ.
43019024	Ka ba 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Yɩ ta ɩ a sɩ chɩɛr a fuu nyã ɛ, yɩ ɩ a sɩ gba gbãm kaa an lɛ na di?" Ba ɩn a lɛ ka a ala na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, "Ba põn a n fuur tɩ de a n fuu gbãn gbãm." Lɛ lɛ a sojasɩ ɩ.
43019025	Yesu ma nɩ a wʋ ma yɛbɛ, Klopasɩ pɔɔ Mɛɛr nɩ a Mɛɛr 'lɔ mɩ na yi a Magdala ara naa be a wʋ daa par.
43019026	A Yesu na nyɛ a wʋ ma na ara, ka a poturo 'lɔ wʋn nʋ̃ mɩ ara gbʋr wʋ, ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a ma, "A fʋ bie lɛ a 'lɔ."
43019027	Na wʋ mɩ 'yɛr kʋ a poturo 'lɔ mɩ, "A fʋ ma lɛ." Ala lɛ so ka a poturo 'lɔ tara a Yesu ma kul a wʋ yir.
43019028	Yesu bɔ̃ɔn naa pʋ̃pãanyã ɩka yele a jaa pãa baar naa ka a lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Kɔ̃nyũur kpɛ ma naa."
43019029	Dʋʋ ben be ka a dãmiir sɛɛ ka ba de sapɔ 'lɔr ir chab urbanyũu daa pɔ tur a Yesu.
43019030	Wʋn wa mʋʋr a dãmiir ala baar, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "A baar naa," tɩ sur a ju na wʋ ŋmaa a vʋʋr.
43019031	A bɩbir chiiraa Chɔɔrfʋ Bɩbir Daar lɛ ka a wɛr na chaar ɩ Bɩbir Kpɛ̃ɛ, ala lɛ so ka a Juu nɩbɛ ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka a kũn a chɛnɛ be a daar jur ɛ. Ba sʋɔr a Pilate ɩka wʋ vɛ̃ ka ba kar a ba gbɛɛ tɩ yɔɔ ba.
43019032	Be lɛ a sojasɩ chen tɩ kar a bala ban lɔ̃ɔ kpan a Yesu gbɛɛ.
43019033	Tɩchɛ ban wa ta a Yesu sɛ̃, ba nyɛn ka a ɩ wʋ kpi naa ka baa kar a wʋ gbɛɛ ɛ.
43019034	Ka a sojasɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ de a pĩi wõo 'lɔ chɔr a Yesu lõboor ka jɩ̃ɩ nɩ kʋ̃ɔ yi ajienaa.
43019035	A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nyɛ a anyãna lɛ di a dãasɩɛ, ka wʋ dãasɩɛ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ. Wʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ, ka yɩ mɩ na sɔɔ de.
43019036	A anyãna ɩ naa ka a lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka, "A wʋ kɔɔr kʋ̃ kab ɛ."
43019037	Ka ba lɛ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn jie ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩka, "Ban kaa naa a 'lɔ ban chɔr."
43019038	A Josefʋ na yi Arimatɩya, ɩ naa a Yesu poturo, tɩ a Juu nɩbɛrɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ jũu, waa dɔ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka ba bɔ̃ɔn ɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ sʋɔr a Yesu a Pilate sɛ̃. Pilate sɔɔ naa ka wʋ tɩ yɔɔ a Yesu.
43019039	A 'lɔ nɩ a Nikodimasɩ nyã na dɔ̃ɔ chen a Yesu sɛ̃ a tɩ̃sɔɔ pʋɔ wʋ naa, na wʋ mɩ waan a kãnyũur ala ban bʋɔlɔ sɩmura nɩ alosɩ. An tãn nũgbulo lɩjaata nɩ pie nɩ a nũu (75).
43019040	A ba jaa ayi den a Yesu vil wʋ a fɔpɩla tɩ jɛ wʋ a kãnyũu ala tu a lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ na ma ɩ tɩ ũu a nɩrɛ.
43019041	A jie 'lɔ ban kpa a Yesu, pobile ben be, ka yaa paalaa mɩ ban ba ũu nɩrɛ jaa ɛ, mɩ be be.
43019042	Bojũu an ɩ a bɩbir chiiraa Chɔɔrfʋ Bɩbir Daar lɛ, tɩchɛ ka a yaa mɩ gbʋr a be jũu, ba ũun a Yesu a be.
43020001	A daa gbul bɩbir dɔ̃ɔ daar wɛr na chaara wa la la la, Mɛɛr na yi a Magdala chen naa a yaa par tɩ nyɛ ka ɩ a kʋsɩr 'lɔ ban pɔɔ a yaa yuo naa.
43020002	Wʋ jon chen a Simon Pita nɩ a poturo 'lɔ a Yesu na nʋ̃ sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "Ba ir naa a Soro ɩ̃gãn a yaa pɔ, ka saa bɔ̃ɔ a jie ban bin wʋ ɛ."
43020003	Ka a Pita nɩ a poturo yi na chen a yaa par.
43020004	Ba jaa 'mantaa joro, tɩchɛ ka a poturo 'lɔ jo vɩɛ a Pita bar tɩ de nie ta a yaa par.
43020005	Na wʋ muul nyɛ a fɔpɩla 'lɔ na gã, tɩ waa kpɛ ɛ.
43020006	Be lɛ ka a Pita na turo a puor mɩ ta, na wʋ kpɛ a yaa pɔ, na wʋ nyɛ a fɔpɩla mɩ na gã.
43020007	Ka a fɔ-ũu naa 'lɔ ban vil a Yesu ju mɩ pil yi a fɔpɩla pɔ gã wʋ yõ.
43020008	A poturo 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ de nie ta a yaa par mɩ pãa kpɛ, na wʋ nyɛ a lɛ tɩ sɔɔ de.
43020009	Baa na bɔ̃ɔ a par sɛrɛ ɛ, ɩka lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr ɩka a Yesu na ir naa a kũu pɔ, ɩ vʋr ɛ.
43020010	A poturbo ayi bala lɩɛb kul a ba taaba sɛ̃.
43020011	Tɩchɛ ka a Mɛɛr ara a yaa par kõnõ. Wʋ kõn wa muul kaa a yaa pɔ,
43020012	na wʋ nyɛ a malakasɩ ayi na su fuu pɩɛl be a yaa pɔ, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ jɩ̃nɛ a ju jie, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ jɩ̃nɛ a gbɛɛ jie, a jie ban dɔ̃ɔ gaal a Yesu.
43020013	Ka ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Pɔɔ, bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ fʋ kõnõ?" A wʋ 'yɛr ba, "Ba ir naa a n Soro, ka n ba bɔ̃ɔ a jie ban bin wʋ ɛ."
43020014	A nɩtɔ̃ wʋn 'yɛr, tɩ lɩɛb nyɛ a Yesu na ara, tɩchɛ waa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɛ.
43020015	Ka Yesu sʋʋr wʋ, "Pɔɔ, bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ fʋ kõnõ? An lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ?" Mɛɛr tɩɛr naa ɩka a jikaara lɛ, tɩ 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ir wʋ, wiil ma a jie fʋn bin, ka n chen tɩ 'mɔɔ wʋ."
43020016	A Yesu bʋɔl, "Mɛɛr!" Ka wʋ lɩɛb 'yɛr nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr, "Woroboni." A par lɛ, Wiwile.
43020017	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Ta gɔɔ ma ɛ, n ba chen a n Sãa sɛ̃ sɛrɛ ɛ. Chen a n poturbo sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr ba, n lɩɛb chiine a n Sãa Nãaŋmɩn mɩ na ɩ a yɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃."
43020018	Ka a Mɛɛr na yi a Magdala chen a poturbo sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "N nyɛn a Soro," na wʋ mɩ man a ala a Yesu na 'yɛr kʋ wʋ.
43020019	A daa gbul bɩbir dɔ̃ɔ daar jãanʋɔr, a poturbo lɔ̃ɔn taa a die pɔ, tɩ kpal a pãma a Juu nɩbɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ jũu. A Yesu tɩ kpɛ ara a ba sɛ̃ tɩ puor ba 'yɛr, "Nyã'maar wʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃."
43020020	Wʋn 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃, wʋ wiil ba naa a nuur nɩ a lõboor. Nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ̃n a poturbo ban nyɛ a Soro.
43020021	Yesu lɛ 'yɛr kʋ ba go, "Nyã'maar wʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃, lɛ a Sãa na tʋ̃ ma, lɛ lɛ n mɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ yɩ."
43020022	Tɩ pãa vʋʋr 'yɔ̃ɔ ba tɩ 'yɛr, "Yɩ de a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ."
43020023	Ala ɩ yɩ vɛ̃n nɩrɛ yeldɛɛr bar, Nãaŋmɩn mɩ na vɛ̃n bar wʋ. Ala ɩ yaa mɩ wa vɛ̃ bar ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn mɩ kʋ̃ vɛ̃ bar ɛ.
43020024	Tomasɩ ban lɛ bʋɔlɔ Naa na ɩ a Poturo Pie Nɩ Ayi ɩ̃sʋɔ ba dɔ̃ɔ be be a Yesu na wa ɛ.
43020025	Ka a poturbo bala na be be nyɛ a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Sɩ nyɛn a Soro," tɩ wʋ 'yɛr, "Maa ba nyɛ a natɩɛ a wʋ nũu pɔ ɛ, naa de a n nubir tũ a kpafʋ jie ɛ, naa mɩ lɛ de nũu tũ a lõboor bɔɔ pɔ ɛ, n kʋ̃ sɔɔ de jaa ɛ."
43020026	A ber aniin daar, a wʋ poturbo ba jaa lɛ lɔ̃ɔn taa a yir pɔ, ka a Tomasɩ mɩ be be. A pãma kpal naa, tɩchɛ ka a Yesu wa ara a ba sɛ̃ puor ba tɩ 'yɛr, "Nyã'maar wʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃."
43020027	Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a Tomasɩ, "Tur a fʋ nubir a ka, nyɛ a n nuur na fʋ tur a fʋ nũu su a n lõboor bɔɔ pɔ, na fʋ bar a baal tɩ sɔɔ de."
43020028	Ka a Tomasɩ 'yɛr, "N Soro nɩ n Nãaŋmɩn."
43020029	A Yesu pãa sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋn nyɛ ma jũu lɛ fʋ sɔɔ de ɔ? Pʋpɛl dẽme lɛ a bala na ba nyɛ ɛ, tɩ sɔɔ de."
43020030	Yesu tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃ yɔɔ a wʋ poturbo niem, ban ba sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ a gãn nyã pɔ ɛ.
43020031	Tɩchɛ a anyãna sɛb naa ka yɩn sɔɔ de ɩka, a Yesu lɛ a Nɩ-iraa, na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie. Yɩn sɔɔ de jũu, yɩn tara naa nyɛvʋr yin a wʋ yuor pɔ.
43021001	A anyã puor, Yesu lɛ ir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ wiil kʋ a wʋ poturbo be a Tiberiyas man pɔ. Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a tu.
43021002	Simon Pita, Tomasɩ ban bʋɔlɔ Naa, Natanɩɛl na yi Keena na be a Galilee paal pɔ, Jebedee bibiir ayi pʋɔn a poturbo ayi bamɩne 'mantaa.
43021003	Ka a Simon Pita 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Maa chiine naa jɩ̃mɛ nyɔɔrfʋ jie." Ka ba mɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩn 'mantaa chen!" Ba yin kpɛ a gboro chen, tɩchɛ a tɩ̃sɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ baa nyɔɔ bon ɛ.
43021004	Bibio pipi Yesu ben a gogoro ju ara, tɩchɛ a poturbo ba bɔ̃ɔ ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɛ.
43021005	Ka wʋ bʋɔl ba sʋʋr, "Barmɩne, yaa nyɔɔ jɩ̃m ɛ?" Ka ba 'yɛr "Kai."
43021006	A Yesu 'yɛr ba, "Yɩ lɔb a lɔyaar 'yɔ̃ɔ a gboro nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, yɩn nyɔɔr amɩne." Ban lɔb a lɔyaar 'yɔ̃ɔ, baa lɛ tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ tɔɔrɔ ɛ, bojũu wʋ nyɔɔr jɩ̃yɔɔ.
43021007	Ka a poturo 'lɔ a Yesu na nʋ̃ 'yɛr kʋ a Simon Pita, "A sɩ Soro lɛ." A lɛ a Pita na wõ ɩka, "A sɩ Soro lɛ," wʋ sun a fuu wʋn dɔ̃ɔ yaa bar na wʋ ɔɔ lon a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ.
43021008	Ka a poturbo ba nyã na chɛ turo nɩ a gboro tɔɔrɔ a lɔyaar na sɛɛn a jɩ̃mɛ. Baa jãan a gogoro ɛ, an ɩn gbɛɛ kɔɔr ata (300).
43021009	Ban wa do a gogoro ju, ba nyɛn saalaa bũu jɩ̃mɛ na be be nɩ paanʋ̃ɔ.
43021010	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ir a jɩ̃mɛ ala yɩn nyɔɔr a pʋ̃pãanyã amɩne waan."
43021011	Ka a Simon Pita kpɛ a gboro pɔ, tɩ tɔɔ a lɔyaar na sɛɛn a jɩ̃bɛrɛ don a gogoro ju. A ɩn jɩ̃mɛ kɔbaa lɩjaayi nɩ pie nɩ ata (153), an ɩ a yɔɔ a lɛ, tɩchɛ a lɔyaar ba chɩɛr ɛ.
43021012	A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ wa suor nɛɛ." Tɩ a poturbo ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba 'la sʋʋr wʋ ɩka, "An lɛ fʋ ɩ?" Ba jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a Soro lɛ.
43021013	Yesu ir a paanʋ̃ɔ na wʋ kʋ ba, tɩ lɛ ir a jɩ̃mɛ mɩ kʋ ba.
43021014	A nyã lɛ ɩ gbɛɛ ata Yesu na ir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ wiil a poturbo wʋn ir a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋr.
43021015	Ban di baar ka Yesu sʋʋr a Simon Pita, "Simon, Jɔɔn bie, fʋ nʋ̃ man gar a banyãna ɔ?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, n Soro, fʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩn nʋ̃ fʋ." A Yesu 'yɛr wʋ, "Kʋrɔ a n pelsɩ a bʋ̃diir."
43021016	Yesu lɛ sʋʋr go, "Simon, Jɔɔn bie, fʋ nʋ̃ man sɩrɛ jaa?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, n Soro, fʋ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩn nʋ̃ fʋ." Ka a Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Bɔ̃ɔ kaara ma a piir."
43021017	Yesu lɛ sʋʋr wʋn gbɛɛ ata, "Simon Jɔɔn bie, fʋ nʋ̃ ma naa?" Ka a Pita pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ bojũu gbɛɛ ata nɩ nyã a Yesu na sʋʋr wʋ, ɩka wʋ, "Nʋ̃ wʋ naa?" Tɩ 'yɛr, "N Soro fʋ bɔ̃ɔn yele a jaa, fʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩn nʋ̃ fʋ." A Yesu 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Kʋrɔ ma a piir bʋ̃diir.
43021018	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, a fʋ pɔlbile daar fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ma sun fʋ fuusɩ na fʋ chiin jie 'lɔ jaa fʋn bʋɔrɔ. Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ wa kor baar, fʋ ma jãn a nuur ka nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ su fʋ a fuu tɩ tɔɔ fʋ chiin a jie 'lɔ fʋn ba bʋɔrɔ ɛ."
43021019	Yesu 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃ na wʋ wiil a kũu 'lɔ tɔ Pita na wa kpi 'yɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn yuor tɩɩr. Tɩ pãa 'yɛr kʋ a Pita, "Turo ma."
43021020	Pita lɩɛb nyɛ a poturo 'lɔ a Yesu na nʋ̃ ka wʋ turo ba. A poturo nyã lɛ dɔ̃ɔ dɩɛl a Yesu lɛ ban dire a di baaraa, na dɔ̃ɔ sʋʋr a Yesu, "N Soro, an lɛ na gar 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ?"
43021021	Pita na nyɛ wʋn turo ba, ka wʋ sʋʋr, "N Soro, tɩ nyã mɩ?"
43021022	A Yesu 'yɛr, "Maa nʋ̃ ɩka wʋ be be tɩ tãn ɩn na lɩɛb wa, a ɩ bo a fʋ sʋrɔ? Fʋ̃ʋ turo ma."
43021023	A anyãna jũu lɛ a poturbo 'yɛr yʋɔrɔ nɩ ɩka a poturo 'lɔ kʋ̃ kpi ɛ. Tɩchɛ Yesu ba 'yɛr ɩka wʋ kʋ̃ kpi ɛ, wʋ 'yɛr ɩka, "Maa nʋ̃ ɩka wʋ be be tɩ tãn ɩn na lɩɛb wa, a ɩ bo a fʋ sʋrɔ?"
43021024	A poturo nyãna lɛ di a anyãna dãasɩɛ na wʋ sɛb bin, ka sɩ bɔ̃ɔn a wʋ dãasɩɛ na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
43021025	Yesu tʋ̃n tʋ̃yɔɔ mɩ, ala ɩ a jaa ta sɛb bʋ̃'yen 'yen, a wɛr wʋ jaa kʋ̃ naa tara jie bin a ala na sɛb ɛ.
44001001	Teofilusɩ a n gãn dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ pɔ, n sɛb a ala a jaa a Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ piel maal tɩ na wʋ wiil a nɩbɛ.
44001002	Yesu tu naa a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pɔ na wʋ wiil a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ bala wʋn ir lɛ ban na ɩrɛ tɩ a Nãaŋmɩn de wʋ don a saaju.
44001003	A wʋ dɔɔyɛ difʋ puor, wʋ wiil wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a nɩbɛ banyãna, ka a chaar ba nie ɩka wʋ ir naa na wʋ ɩ vʋr. A ber lɩjaayi daar lɛ wʋ wa dũu ba, na wʋ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr.
44001004	Wʋn wa lɔ̃ɔn ba ka ba 'mataa dire, ka wʋ kpãkpãan ba nɩ a 'yɛr bir nyã, "Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa yire a Jerusalɛm ɛ, yɩ chɛlɛ a kʋfʋ 'lɔ a n Sãa na põl ka n 'yɛr kʋ yɩ.
44001005	Jɔɔn 'lɔ, kʋ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ de son a nɩbɛ, tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ, a kʋ̃ lɛ kor ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn na so yɩ naa nɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ."
44001006	Ba lɛ wa lɔ̃ɔn naa a Yesu go, na ba sʋʋr wʋ, "Sɩ Soro, a sɔ̃ɔ nyãna pɔ lɛ fʋn lɩɛb a Isɩral nãalʋ̃ʋ kʋ ba bɩɩ?"
44001007	A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A ba ɩ yɩ 'yɛr ɛ, ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a sɔ̃ɔ bɩɩ a bɩbir a Sãa na bin a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ ɛ.
44001008	Tɩchɛ yɩn nyɛn kpɛ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wa wa a yɩ sɛ̃, ka yɩ ɩ a n dãasɩɛ dẽme, a Jerusalɛm, nɩ a Judiya paal wʋ jaa, nɩ a Samariya paal tɩ tãn a wɛr tɛɛfʋ jie."
44001009	A anyãna lɛ wʋ 'yɛr baar tɩ duoro a saaju a lɛ nɛ a ba nɩbiru ka a julõjuur tɩ pɔɔ wʋ.
44001010	Ka ba chɛnɛ dʋl kaara a saaju a lɛ nɛ wʋn duoro, be lɛ a dɔɔr ayi na su fuu pɩɛl wa dũu ba a lɛ nɛ ara a ba sɛ̃.
44001011	Na ba sʋʋr ba, "Galilee dɔɔr, bãa lɛ so a yɩ kaara a saaju a lɛ mɔ̃? A Yesu nyãna nɩ wʋ ju yɩn nyɛ na duoro a saaju, na lɩɛb a lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju wa, nɩtãa a lɛ nɛ yɩn nyɛ wʋn duoro a saaju."
44001012	A ba yi a tɔ̃ɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Olive Tɩɩr Tɔ̃ɔ lɩɛb kul a Jerusalɛm na ba jãan a tẽe ɛ, a fʋn tʋ̃ɔ chen a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar.
44001013	Ban wa ta, ba don a bɔɔpɩɛ pɔ, be lɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ lɔ̃ɔ taa. Ka a bala na dɔ̃ɔ be be lɛ Pita, Jɔɔn, Jemesɩ nɩ Andiru. Filip, Tomasɩ, Batolomi nɩ Matiu nɩ Alfayasɩ bidaba Jemesɩ nɩ Simon na mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a wʋ wɛr yele, nɩ a Jemesɩ bidaba Judas.
44001014	A banyãna ba jaa lɛ lɔ̃ɔ taa nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn, ka a pɔbɔ bamɩne pʋɔ ba ka a Yesu yɛɛr nɩ a wʋ ma Mɛɛr mɩ be be.
44001015	Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ a wʋ poturbo wa lɔ̃ɔ taa na ba ɩ nɩbɛ kɔbaa dɔɔl lɩjɛr. Ka Pita ir ara a ba pɔ
44001016	tɩ 'yɛr, "Yɛɛr, a sɛɛ naa ka sɩn maal a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na dɔ̃ɔ tu a Nãa David nɛɛ pɔ, a wʋ 'yɛr na wʋ sɛb bin a kõr jaa nɩtãa lɛ a Judas nyã na dɔ̃ɔ de a nɩbɛ nie a ba wa nyɔɔ a Yesu.
44001017	Wʋ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na wʋ pʋɔ sɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ nyã pɔ."
44001018	Judas putuyar wʋn nyɛ lɛ ɩka wʋ dãn wɛr, be lɛ wʋ chʋr ju pur ka a nyaba a jaa yi.
44001019	Nɩrɛ jaa na be ka a Jerusalɛm lɛ wõ a 'yɛr nyã na ba bʋɔlɔ a jie a ba kɔkɔr pɔ ɩka, Akeldama. A par lɛ, Jɩ̃ɩ Wɛr.
44001020	Ka a Pita 'yɛr, "Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Nãa David sɛb a wʋ yiel gãn pɔ, 'A wʋ jie wʋ lɩɛb dãlpʋɔ, ka a nɩrɛ jaa taa kpɩɛrɛ be ɛ,' ka, 'A nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ, wʋ de a wʋ jie.'
44001021	"A lɛ jũu, nɩyuo lɛ sɩn ir ka a nɩnyɩnɛ ɩ a 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ pʋɔ sɩ 'mataa yʋɔrɔ nɩ a Yesu.
44001022	Piel a Jɔɔn Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ sɔ̃ɔ wa tãn a sɔ̃ɔ nyã a Yesu na yi a sɩ sɛ̃ do a saaju. A nɩrɛ 'lɔ lɛ na pʋɔ sɩ dire a wʋ kũu pɔ irfʋ dãasɩɛ."
44001023	Be lɛ ba tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩbɛ ayi. Josefʋ ban bʋɔlɔ Basabasɩ na ba lɛ bʋɔlɔ wʋ Jusɩtusɩ nɩ Matɩyasɩ.
44001024	Na ba pãa sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ, "Sɩ Soro, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ jaa pʋtɩɛr, wiil sɩ a nɩbɛ ayi banyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ fʋn na ir.
44001025	Ka wʋn de a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ jie a Judas na bar, tɩ chen a jie wʋn pʋɔ."
44001026	A ba pãa gba gbãm ka a gbãbie tɩ ir Matɩyasɩ a wʋ pʋɔ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ pie nɩ bʋ̃'yen pɔ.
44002001	A Pentikosɩ na wa ta, ba jaa ben a jibʋ̃'yen.
44002002	Ajienaa lɛ ka a damfʋ na kaara fɩka sɛsɛkpɛ̃ɛ na furo yi a saaju wa sɛɛ a die 'lɔ pɔ ban jɩ̃nɛ.
44002003	Be lɛ ba nyɛ bũu 'lɩraa na ŋmara jaa pʋrpʋr dɔɔlɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa bʋ̃'yen 'yenɩ.
44002004	Ka ba jaa sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na ba piel 'yɛrɛ kɔkɔyor lɛ a Sɩɛ na kʋ ba.
44002005	A Juu nɩbɛ na joro a Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ na ba yi a tẽn tẽn wa kpɩɛrɛ a be a Jerusalɛm.
44002006	Ban wa wõ a gɔ̃mɔ̃ nyã, a nɩyɔɔ ba nyãna ba jaa wa lɔ̃ɔn taa na ba ɩ chĩcham, bojũu ɩ̃sʋɔ ma wõn ban 'yɛrɛ a wʋ kɔkɔr.
44002007	Ka a ɩ yel dũu naa, na a 'maa ba jaa nɛɛ ka ba sʋrɔ taa, "A ba ɩ Galilee dẽme lɛ a banyãna na 'yɛrɛ ɛ?
44002008	Tɩ ŋmɩnɛ a ɩ ka a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wõnõ ban 'yɛrɛ nɩ a sɩ kɔkɔɛ?
44002009	Parti dẽme, Mede dẽme, nɩ a Elam dẽme. Bamɩne mɩ yin Mesopotamiya, Judiya, Kapadosiya nɩ Pontus nɩ Asɩya.
44002010	Ka bamɩne mɩ yi Fɩrgɩya, nɩ Pamfiliya, nɩ Ijipitɩ, nɩ a Libiya dẽme na gbʋr a Sirenɩ wɛr nɩ a sãanba na yi a Worom,
44002011	a Juu nɩbɛ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bala na lɩɛb a Juu nɩbɛ, bamɩne yin Kɩrete nɩ a Arabɩya dẽme. Sɩ wõn ban de a sɩ mɩ̃ɛ kɔkɔr 'yɛrɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃bɛrɛ wʋn tʋ̃."
44002012	Ka a anyãna sɔb ba nɩbir ka ba nɛɛr 'maa a ba sʋrɔ taa, "A anyãna par nɩ bo?"
44002013	Tɩchɛ ka a bamɩne kpɛrɛ 'yɛrɛ, "Dãa lɛ maal ba a lɛ nɛ."
44002014	Ka a Pita nɩ a Pie Nɩ Bʋ̃'yen pãa ir ara ka wʋ 'yɛr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa kʋ a nɩbɛ, "Juu nɩbɛ nɩ nɩrɛ jaa na kpɩɛrɛ ka a Jerusalɛm, yɩ vɛ̃ ka n wiil yɩ a par. Yɩ chɛlɛ a lɛ ɩn na 'yɛr.
44002015	A nɩbɛ banyãna ba nyũ dãa ɛ, nɩtãa a lɛ yɩn tɩɛr ɛ, a chɛnɛ na ɩ bibi'maar.
44002016	Nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Joɛl dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr,
44002017	'Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɩka a ber baaraa daar, wʋn kpaaraa a wʋ Sɩɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɩbɛ ba jaa. Ka a yɩ dabil nɩ a pɔɔbil 'yɛrɛ a 'yɛrsɩ ala a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ ba, ka a yɩ dabil nyɛrɛ nyɛfʋsɩ, ka a yɩ danyɔ̃n mɩ jãna jãnsɩ.
44002018	A bala gba na ɩ a n gbãgbadɔɔr nɩ a pɔbɔ, ba jaa pɔ lɛ ɩn kpaar a n Sɩɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba a ber ala pɔ, ka ba 'yɛrɛ a n 'yɛr.
44002019	Ɩn wiil ban yelfɛrsɩ na yi saaju ka a jɩ̃nsɩ mɩ be ka a tẽe, jɩ̃ɩ, bũu nɩ jʋʋr na den jie wʋ jaa.
44002020	Ka a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ lɩɛb lĩi ka a ŋmɛra mɩ lɩɛb jɩ̃ɩ kaar tɩchɛ ka a sɩ Soro bɩbir 'lɔn na chaar pãa wa.
44002021	Be lɛ nɩrɛ jaa na pãa bʋɔlɔ a sɩ Soro yuor na nyɛn faafʋ.'
44002022	"Isɩral nɩbɛ yɩ chɛlɛ ka, A Yesu nyã na yi a Najaretɩ 'lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn ir kʋ yɩ, na wʋ de wʋ tʋ̃n a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃, nɩ tʋ̃fɛrsɩ, nɩ jɩ̃nsɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ a yɩ pɔ, ka yɩ mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn.
44002023	Ba nyɔɔn a daba nyãna 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩ nuur pɔ nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ tu a wʋ bɔfʋ nɩ a wʋ bɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ, de nie 'yɛr bin, ka a putudẽme sʋ̃ʋ yɩ ka yɩ kpa wʋ a daa ju a wʋ kpi.
44002024	Tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a kũu pɔ, na wʋ faa wʋ a kũu wõm pɔ, bojũu a kũu ba tara kpɛ̃ɔ na nyɔɔ wʋ taa lɛ ɛ.
44002025	"A Nãa David dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr, 'Bɩbir jaa lɛ n nyɛrɛ a n Soro, bojũu wʋ ben a n nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, n kʋ̃ wa lɔɔ gbɛr ɛ.
44002026	Ala lɛ so ka n pʋɔ pɛl ka n jãlbir chɩlɛ, ka a n ɩ̃gãn mɩ tara tɩɛr tɔfʋ jie.
44002027	Bojũu fʋ kʋ̃ wa bar ma be a yaa pɔ ɛ, bɩɩ ka fʋ bar a fʋ Chɛchɛ Sʋɔ 'lɔ ka wʋ pʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
44002028	Fʋ wiil man a nyɛvʋr sɔr, fʋn vɛ̃n ka nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ma a fʋ niem.'
44002029	"N yɛɛr, n 'yɛr chãa pɔ kʋ yɩ ɩka a sɩ sãakpã David kpi naa a ba ũu, a wʋ yaa lɛ anyãna na be ka dɩna.
44002030	Tɩchɛ wʋ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr nɛɛ kʋ wʋ ɩka, wʋn vɛ̃ naa ka 'lɔ David yɔ̃ɔ jɩ̃nɛ a wʋ nãa dakɔɔ ju.
44002031	David den nie nyɛ a lɛ na be a wʋ niem, ala lɛ so ka wʋ 'yɛr a Kɩrɩsɩto kũu pɔ irfʋ 'yɛr, na wʋ 'yɛr ɩka wʋ kʋ̃ gã be a yaa pɔ ɛ, bɩɩ ka a wʋ ɩ̃gãn pʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
44002032	"Nãaŋmɩn sɩ̃ɩ naa a Yesu nyãna ka wʋ ir ɩ vʋr, sɩn lɛ ɩ a anyãna a jaa dãasɩɛ dẽme.
44002033	'Lɔ lɛ wʋ 'mɔɔ don bin a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, ka a Sãa kʋ a Yesu a wʋ Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ wʋ. A Sɩɛ nyã lɛ wʋ kpaar 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ ka yɩ nyɛ tɩ be wõnõ.
44002034	David ba dɔ̃ɔ do a saaju ɛ, tɩ wʋ 'yɛr naa, 'A Soro 'yɛr kʋ a n Soro, "Jɩ̃nɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ jie,
44002035	ka n wa de a fʋ dɔ̃dẽme ka ba ɩ a fʋ gbɛɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie." '
44002036	"A lɛ jũu, vɛ̃ ka a Isɩral nɩbɛ ba jaa bɔ̃ɔ sɩrɛ jaa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn maal naa Yesu nyã yɩn kpa a daa ju ka wʋ ɩ a sɩ Soro nɩ a Nɩ-iraa."
44002037	A nɩbɛ na wõ a nɩtɔ̃, ka a ŋmara ba a nyãn, ka ba sʋʋr a Pita nɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ, "N yɛɛr, ŋmɩnɛ sɩn ɩ?"
44002038	Ka a Pita 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr, ka ba de a Yesu yuor son yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ka a yɩ yelbier baar. Ka a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ yɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ.
44002039	Yɩn nɩ a yɩ bibiir lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ kʋ, yɩn nɩ a bala ba jaa na be a tɛɛr, nɩ a bala ba jaa a sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn na wa bʋɔl."
44002040	Pita den 'yɛr yɔɔ kpãan ba, na wʋ kpãkpãan ba 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩ faa yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin a dɩna nɩfɩlefɩlesɩ pɔ."
44002041	Ka a bala na sɔɔ de a wʋ 'yɛr, ba so naa a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ka nɩbɛ tur ata (3,000) pʋɔ ba a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
44002042	Ba den ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ wiilfʋ, na ba tara nɛbʋ̃'yen lɔ̃ɔ dire, na ba lɔ̃ɔ puoro a Nãaŋmɩn.
44002043	Dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ̃n nɩrɛ jaa a lɛ ban nyɛ ka a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ tʋ̃ a tʋ̃fɛrsɩ nɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃.
44002044	A bala na sɔɔ de, ba jaa lɔ̃ɔn taa jibʋ̃'yen na ba sʋ̃nɔ̃ taa.
44002045	Na ba daara a ba bʋ̃tarsɩ na ba ma põ ir kʋ taa lɛ jaa ɩ̃sʋɔ na bʋɔrɔ.
44002046	Bɩbir jaa lɛ ba ma lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, na ba yʋɔrɔ taa yie ŋmara a paanʋ̃ɔ dire nɩ pʋpɛl nɩ pʋtɩɛr bʋ̃'yen.
44002047	Ba pɛɛrɛ naa Nãaŋmɩn ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa mɩ ara a ba puor. A sɩ Soro ma vɛ̃ naa ka a bala na nyɛ faafʋ, pʋɔ ba bɩbir jaa.
44003001	Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ Pita nɩ Jɔɔn duoro naa a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ, a puorfʋ jie mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na gɔr.
44003002	Ka a daba ban lɔ̃ɔ dɔɔn a wʋ gbɛr, a ba ma tuo wʋ tɩ bin a be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ, Vɩla. Be lɛ ba ma tuo wʋ tɩ bin bɩbir jaa a wʋ ma sʋɔrɔ a bala na kpɩɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn yir bɛchaar pɔ libie.
44003003	Wʋn wa nyɛ a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn na kpɩɛrɛ, a wʋ sʋɔrɔ ba a libir.
44003004	Ka a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn kaara wʋ a lɛ a tɩ̃ɩɩ, ka a Pita wa 'yɛr, "Kaara sɩ."
44003005	Ka a daba tɔ̃ɔ fur a nɩbir a lɛ chir chir chir 'yɔ̃ɔ ba tɩɛrɛ ɩka wʋn nyɛn bon.
44003006	A Pita pãa 'yɛr, "N ba tara libir bɩɩ, sɛlma kʋrɔ fʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ ɩn tara lɛ ɩn kʋ fʋ. Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na yi a Najaretɩ yuor pɔ, ir chiine."
44003007	Tɩ na wʋ nyɔɔ a daba nũsʋ̃ɔ sʋ̃ʋ wʋ ka wʋ ir ka a ɩ a gbɛpɛlɛ nɩ a nakɔɔtɩɛ kpɛ̃mɛ naa.
44003008	Ka a daba ɔɔ chʋr a gbɛɛ na wʋ piel chiine, na wʋ pãa tu ba kpɛ̃n be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ. Be lɛ wʋ tɩ ɔɔrɔ yʋɔrɔ na wʋ pɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn.
44003009	A nɩbɛ ba jaa na wa nyɛ wʋ, a lɛ wʋn chiine pɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn,
44003010	ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa an ɩ 'lɔ lɛ ma jɩ̃nɛ sʋɔrɔ libie be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir dɔ̃dɔr 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a, Vɩla. Ka a ɩ ba chĩcham naa 'maa ba nɛɛ a lɛ na ɩ.
44003011	An ɩ a daba chɛnɛ na pɔɔ a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn ka a nɩbɛ nɛɛr 'maa a ba jo wa titaa a be ban bʋɔlɔ a Solomon Bɛchaar pɔ.
44003012	Pita na nyɛ a lɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ, "Isɩral dɔɔr woɩ, bãa lɛ so ka a nɛɛr 'maa yɩ a lɛ mɔ̃? Bãa lɛ yɩ fur a nɩbir 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ fɩka sɩn mɩ̃ɛ kpɛ̃ɔ bɩɩ sɩn mɩ̃ɛ maal vɩla lɛ sɩ maal a daba nyã ka wʋ chiine?
44003013	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ a Abraham, Isaakɩ nɩ a Jekɔb Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne Nãaŋmɩn lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ Yesu yuor. Yɩn lɛ nyɔɔ wʋ tɩr ɩka ba kʋ wʋ, ka a Pilate ŋme nyãa na bar wʋ tɩ yɩ 'yɛr ɩka yaa bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ.
44003014	Yɩ 'yɛr naa ɩka yaa bɔ̃ɔ a chɛchɛ sʋɔ nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ ɛ, tɩ na yɩ sʋɔr ka ba yuo a nɩkʋrɔ kʋ yɩ.
44003015	Yɩn lɛ kʋ a nyɛvʋr sʋɔ, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a kũu pɔ. Sɩn lɛ nyɛ anyãna nɩ nɩbir.
44003016	A daba nyãna nɩ a sɩn na 'mataa sɔɔ a Yesu lɛ sa a daba nyãna baal yɩn nyɛ na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ, sɩrɛ jaa sɩn sɔɔ de a Yesu yuor lɛ wʋ sa, a daba nyãna yɩn ben nyɛ.
44003017	"Pʋ̃pãanyã, yɛɛr, n bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka ba bɔ̃ɔ fʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka yɩ tʋ̃ a lɛ nɛ a yɩ nɩbɛrɛ na dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃.
44003018	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn ɩ naa a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ 'yɛr ɩka, a wʋ Nɩ-iraa na din dɔɔyɛ.
44003019	Yɩ pãa lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr, na yɩ lɩɛb wa a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, ka wʋ fɩɛl a yɩ yeldɛbɛ bar. A ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ paalaa yɩn na nyɛ na yin a sɩ Soro sɛ̃,
44003020	ka wʋ gba na tʋ̃ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'lɔ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ ir bin kʋ yɩ.
44003021	Wʋn chɛnɛ na jɩ̃nɛ be a saaju, tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ Nãaŋmɩn na 'mataa a bonsɩ a jaa nɩtãa lɛ wʋn tɩr a nɛɛ a kõr jaa tu, a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ chɛchɛsɩ sɛ̃.
44003022	Bojũu Mosesɩ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, 'A Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ir 'yɛ'yɛrɛ a n kaar ka wʋ ɩ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ nɩrɛ, a yɩ chɛlɛ a ala a jaa wʋn na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ.
44003023	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba wa chɛlɛ a lɛ wʋn na 'yɛrɛ ɛ, ban ir wʋ nũu bar a wʋ nɩbɛ pɔ.'
44003024	"Sɩrɛ jaa, a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ba jaa na yi a Samuwɛl sɔ̃ɔ mɩ 'yɛr naa a bɩbie anyãna 'yɛr.
44003025	Yɩn lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ banyãna bibiir nɩ a nɛtɩraa 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na tara nɩ a sɩ sãamɩne. Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Abraham, 'An tu naa a fʋ yɔn pɔ, ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa na be ka a tẽe na nyɛ sʋ̃ʋfʋ.'
44003026	Nãaŋmɩn na wa ir a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃, yɩn sɛ̃ lɛ wʋ de nie tʋ̃ wʋ ka wʋ tɩ sʋ̃ʋ yɩ na wʋ lɩɛb a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa yin a wʋ putusɔr pɔ."
44004001	A lɛ a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn na chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛ, a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlorbo nɩ a puorfʋ yir nɩdiere 'matãan a Saduseemɩne wan a ba sɛ̃.
44004002	Ba wa nyɛn suur, bojũu ba wile naa a nɩbɛ ɩka Yesu jũu nɩrɛ jaa na ir naa kũu pɔ.
44004003	Be lɛ ba nyɔɔ a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn na ba 'yɔ̃ɔ ba pɔɔfʋ die pɔ bar ka wɛr na chaar, bojũu mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ mʋr baar.
44004004	Tɩchɛ a bala na wõ a lɛ a Pita na 'yɛr a Yesu 'yɛr na ba sɔɔ de na ɩn dɔɔr tur anũu (5,000).
44004005	A wɛr na wa chaar, a ba nɩdierbe nɩ a ba nɩbɛrɛ 'matãan a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe lɔ̃ɔn taa be a Jerusalɛm.
44004006	Ka Anasɩ na ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ Kayafasɩ, Jɔɔn nɩ Aleksanda 'matãan a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩbɛ bamɩne.
44004007	A ba tɩ yuo a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn waan a ba wa sʋrɔ ba, "Kpɛ̃ɔ buor nɩ yobuor lɛ yɩ de tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a anyãna?"
44004008	Ka a Pita na sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A yɩn nɩdierbe nɩ a yɩn nɩbɛrɛ,
44004009	ala ɩ yɩ ben bʋɔl sɩ dɩna ɩka sɩ wa man a maal vɩla nyã na vɛ̃ ka a gbɛrɛ sa.
44004010	Yɩ pãa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka yaa, a yɩn nɩ nɩrɛ jaa na be a Isɩral, ɩka a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nyã na yi a Najaretɩ yuor pɔ, a 'lɔ yɩn kʋ a daa ju, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a kũu pɔ, ka wʋ ɩ vʋr, lɛ sa a daba nyãna na ben ara a kana.
44004011	Wʋ ɩ naa 'A kʋsɩr 'lɔ a yɩn mɩmɩɛrbɛ na tɔr bar, 'lɔ lɛ wa ɩ a kʋsɩr ju.'
44004012	Fafaara jaa ba lɛ be be ɛ, bojũu yuor jaa ba lɛ be ka a tẽe pɔ, na tʋ̃ɔ nɩrɛ faa ɛ."
44004013	Ban nyɛ a lɛ a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn na ba joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩ mɩ bɔ̃ɔn ban ba jãn gãn chen tɛɛr ɛ, ka nɛ'maa ba. Ka ba tɩɛrtɔ ban dɔ̃ɔ be a Yesu sɛ̃.
44004014	Tɩchɛ ba mɩ nyɛn a daba 'lɔ na sa 'mataa ara nɩ ba, baa lɛ tara 'yɛr na 'yɛr ɛ.
44004015	Lɛ lɛ ba 'yɛr ba a ba yi chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ, tɩ ba pãa guoro taa 'yɛrɛ,
44004016	"Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ sɩn ɩ a nɩbɛ banyãna? Nɩrɛ jaa na be ka a Jerusalɛm bɔ̃ɔn naa a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ ban tʋ̃ a sɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ chiir ɛ.
44004017	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ sɩn pɔɔ naa a yele nyãna sɔr ka nɩrɛ kʋ̃ lɛ wõ naa ɛ, yɩ ɩ a sɩ fuu ba ka ba taa ɩrɛ wa pʋrɔ a yuor nyãna kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ."
44004018	Be lɛ ba bʋɔl ba a ba kpɛ ka ba kpãkpãan ba ɩka, ba taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ bɩɩ wile nɩ a Yesu yuor go ɛ.
44004019	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ yɩ pɛ kaa, a sɛɛn Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ka sɩn tu a yɩ nɛɛ gar a Nãaŋmɩn bɩɩ?
44004020	Bojũu sɩn 'lɔ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bar a 'yɛr sɩn nyɛn nɩbir tɩ wõ 'yɛrfʋ ɛ."
44004021	Lɛ lɛ ba vuur ba tɩ bar ba a ba chen. Baa bɔ̃ɔ kpãa buor lɛ ban kpãa ba ɛ, bojũu a nɩbɛ ba jaa pɛɛrɛ naa Nãaŋmɩn a lɛ na ɩ.
44004022	Bojũu a daba nyãna na sa a nɛ'maa safʋ nyãna kor gar yuomo lɩjaayi (40).
44004023	Ban wa bar a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn, ba chen a ba taaba sɛ̃ tɩ man ala a jaa a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ na 'yɛr kʋ ba.
44004024	A ba taaba na wõ a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃, ba jaa 'mantaa nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen puor Nãaŋmɩn na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ Sʋɔ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ maal a saaju nɩ a tẽe nɩ a man kpɛ̃ɛ nɩ bon jaa na be a pɔ.
44004025	Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka a fʋ Sɩɛ haa a fʋ gbãgbaa na ɩ a sɩ sãa David nɛɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr, 'Bo lɛ so ka a paalsɩ nyɛ suur, ka a nɩbɛ ŋmara a dɔɔl pɔrsɩ?
44004026	A wɛr nãmɩne tʋɔrɔ naa gbɛchile, ka a nɩbɛrɛ mɩ lɔ̃ɔ taa jɛɛrɛ nɩ a Soro nɩ a fʋ Nɩ-iraa.'
44004027	Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ a Hɛrɔd nɩ a Pontius Pilate lɔ̃ɔ taa nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ a tẽe nyãna pɔ, na ba jɛb a fʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃chɛchɛ Yesu, a 'lɔ fʋn ir.
44004028	Ba maal naa a lɛ fʋn kaa ir na ɩ a fʋ pʋtɩɛr, nɩ a fʋ kpɛ̃ɔ, nɩ a fʋ bɔfʋ fʋn dɔ̃ɔ de nie chɔɔr tɩ a wa ɩ.
44004029	"Pʋ̃pãanyã sɩ Soro, kaa lɛ ban fuu sɩ, tɩ na fʋ sʋ̃ʋ a fʋ gbãgbaar a sɩ mʋɔl a fʋ 'yɛr nɩ 'lafʋ.
44004030	Tur a fʋ nũu sãan baalsɩ, na fʋ tʋ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ a fʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃chɛchɛ Yesu yuor."
44004031	Ban wa puor baar, a jie 'lɔ ban lɔ̃ɔ taa damaa. Ka ba jaa sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ, na ba 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nɩ 'lafʋ.
44004032	Ka a bala na sɔɔ de, ba jaa tara na tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen nɩ nyãbʋ̃'yen. Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa maa 'yɛr ɩka a wʋ bonsɩ ɩ naa a 'lɔ tɛɛ bon ɛ, ba ma põn bon jaa ban tara.
44004033	A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ den kpɛ̃ɔ mana nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu kũu pɔ irfʋ 'yɛr, ka a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ be a ba jaa sɛ̃.
44004034	Ba ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba dɔ̃ɔ faa bon ɛ, sɔ̃ɔ jaa lɛ a bala na tara por nɩ yie ma da na ba ma waan a libie,
44004035	wa bin a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ sɛ̃, ka ba ma põ ir kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa lɛ an sɛɛn wʋ.
44004036	Josefʋ na yi Sipurusɩ na wʋ ɩ a Levi bal nɩrɛ, kaa a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ bʋɔlɔ wʋ Banabasɩ. A par lɛ nɩrɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
44004037	Wʋ dãn a wʋ puo, na wʋ de a libie waan wa bin a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ sɛ̃.
44005001	Ka a daba ɩ̃sʋɔ na be be di Ananias ka a wʋ pɔɔ mɩ di Safira. Ba mɩ den a ba pobile da.
44005002	Wʋ ir naa libie amɩne bin ka a pɔɔ bɔ̃ɔn, tɩchɛ na wʋ chiin a ŋmaa tɩ bin a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ sɛ̃.
44005003	Ka a Pita sʋʋr a Ananias, "Bo lɛ so ka a Satan sɛɛ fʋ a nyãa a fʋ ŋmaa jir kara yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ, na fʋ ir a libie amɩne a lɛ fʋn da a puo bin?
44005004	A ba ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ so na fʋ de da ɛ? Fʋn wa da baar a ba ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ so a libie ɛ? Bo lɛ ɩ a fʋ tɩɛr a fʋ maal a nɩtɔ̃? Nɩrɛ ba lɛ fʋ ŋmaa a jir nyã 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ."
44005005	Ananias na wõ a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ na wʋ lo kpi a jie. Ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a bala jaa na wõ naa.
44005006	Ka a pɔlbil ir a ba pɔ 'mɔɔ a kũu lũ tuo yin tɩ ũu.
44005007	An wa kor bɩ̃lãa ka a wʋ pɔɔ mɩ wa bʋ̃n dɔɔl ba bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ na ɩ ɛ,
44005008	ka a Pita sʋʋr a pɔɔ, "A libie a jaa lɛ a anyãna a fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a Ananias na da a puo nyɛ ɔ? 'Yɛr kʋ ma." A wʋ 'yɛr, "Ɔ̃ɔ, lɛ lɛ."
44005009	A Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a ɩ a yɩ guor taa ɩka yɩ bɛɛr a sɩ Soro Sɩɛ kaa? Nyɛ a nɩbɛ bala a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ bala lɛ tuo a fʋ sɩrɛ yin tɩ ũu, ba mɩn tuo fʋn yin."
44005010	Ajienaa ka a ɩ wʋ mɩ lon kpi be a Pita niem. A pɔlbil bala na ben wa kpɛ nyɛ ka a ɩ wʋ kpi naa, ka ba tuo wʋ yin tɩ ũu lan a sɩrɛ.
44005011	Ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a pupuorbiir ba jaa nɩ nɩrɛ jaa na wõ naa.
44005012	A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃ yɔɔ a nɩbɛ sɔ̃ɔ. Ka a bala na sɔɔ de, ba jaa tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen ma lɔ̃ɔ taa a be a Solomon Bɛchaar pɔ.
44005013	Nɩrɛ jaa kpire ba naa, tɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa maa 'la lɔ̃ɔn ba ɛ.
44005014	Tɩchɛ nɩyɔɔ jaa chɛnɛ na waara, ka dɔɔr nɩ pɔbɔ na sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro pʋɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
44005015	A lɛ vɛ̃ naa ka a nɩbɛ yin a ba baalsɩ tɩ gaal ba a gador ju nɩ a sɔ̃n pɔ a sɔr kõkoor chɛlɛ nɩ a Pita, ɩka 'lɔ wa tala a wʋ gãagiel wʋ pɔɔ ba.
44005016	Nɩyɔɔ yin a tẽbil ala na jilʋ̃ a Jerusalɛm waan a ba baalsɩ wa lɔ̃ɔn 'matãan a bala a sɩdɛbɛ na tara, ka ba jaa sa.
44005017	Ka a nyuur kpɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a wʋ taaba bala na pʋɔ a Saduseemɩne gbul pɔ.
44005018	A ba nyɔɔr a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ pɔɔfʋ die pɔ bar.
44005019	Tɩchɛ a tɩ̃sɔɔ a sɩ Soro tʋ̃ naa a wʋ malaka ka wʋ wa yuo a pɔɔfʋ die pãn na wʋ tɔɔ ba yin
44005020	tɩ 'yɛr, "Yɩ chen a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ na yɩ tɩ 'yɛr a nyɛvʋr paalaa nyã 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ."
44005021	A wɛr na wa chaar ba kpɛ̃n be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a malaka na 'yɛr ba tɩ piel wile a nɩbɛ. A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a wʋ taaba mɩ wa lɔ̃ɔn taa na ba bʋɔl a Juu nɩbɛ nɩdierbe ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa na ba na guor a 'yɛr, na ba pãa tʋ̃ ɩka ba chen a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ tɩ yuo a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ waan.
44005022	Tɩchɛ ban wa tɩ ta a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ baa nyɛ nɩrɛ jaa ɛ. A ba lɩɛb chen tɩ mana kʋrɔ ba,
44005023	"Sɩ chen tɩ nyɛ a pɔɔfʋ die dɔ̃dɔr na chɛnɛ kpal, ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ara gu chɛnɛ ara a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ, tɩchɛ sɩn wa yuo a pãn nɩrɛ jaa ba be be a die pɔ ɛ."
44005024	Ban wa wõ a anyãna ban man ka a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir guguro nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãmɩne ka a ɩ ba chĩcham, a ba baala baa bɔ̃ɔ lɛn na ɩ ɛ.
44005025	Ka a nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ wa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ nyɛ a nɩbɛ bala yɩn nyɔɔr pɔɔ, ba ben be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ wile a nɩbɛ."
44005026	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir guguro nɩkpɛ̃ɛ tara a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ chiin tɩ tara a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ jaa jom waan. Baa tɩ fɩr ba ɛ, bojũu ba joro na dãbɩ̃ɛ ɩka a nɩbɛ na lɔb ban nɩ kʋsɩbɛ.
44005027	Ban wa waan ba, ba vɛ̃n ka ba ara a nɩbɛrɛ niem, ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na sʋʋr ba 'yɛr,
44005028	"Saa kpãkpãan yɩ jaa 'yɛr ɩka, yɩ taa lɛ ɩrɛ wa pʋrɔ a yuor nyãna wile nɩ nɩrɛ jaa go ɛ? Tɩchɛ a yɩ chɛnɛ tɔr tɩ sɛɛ a Jerusalɛm nɩ a yɩ wiilfʋ nyãna, na yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ de a daba nyãna jɩ̃ɩ yele dɔɔl sɩ."
44005029	Ka a Pita nɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ bala na chɛ 'yɛr, "Sɩn tun Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ gar nɩsaal.
44005030	A sɩ sãakpãmɩne Nãaŋmɩn lɛ sɩ̃ɩ a Yesu a kũu pɔ, a 'lɔ yɩn yɔɔl a daa ju ka wʋ kpi.
44005031	Nãaŋmɩn 'mɔɔ wʋn don bin be a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, ka wʋ ɩ Nãa nɩ Fafaara ɩka wʋ kʋ a Isɩral nɩbɛ sɔr ka ba lɩɛb ba tɩɛr, na ba nyɛ vɛ̃ kʋfʋ.
44005032	Sɩn lɛ ɩ a anyãna dãasɩɛ dẽme nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn de kʋ a bala na tu a wʋ nɛɛ."
44005033	Ban wa wõ a anyãna, ba suur ir naa ka ba bʋɔrɔ a ba kʋfʋ.
44005034	Tɩchɛ ka a Farasee ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Gamaliel na ɩ a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ wiwile, nɩrɛ jaa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ naa, ka wʋ ir ara a nɩdierbe pɔ tɩ 'yɛr ɩka, ba vɛ̃ ka a dɔɔr bala yi yõo bɩ̃lãa.
44005035	Tɩ na wʋ pãa 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Isɩral dɔɔr, yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃ a lɛ yɩn bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ maal a nɩbɛ banyãna.
44005036	Sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Tiudasɩ dɔ̃ɔ ir 'yɛr gãdaa 'yɛr ɩka nɩkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ ka a dɔɔr kɔɔr anaar (400) ir turo wʋ. Ba kʋ wʋ naa ka a nɩbɛ bala yɛ̃yɛl ka a jaa ɩ pɔrɔ.
44005037	Ala puor lɛ ka a Judas na yi a Galilee a nɩbɛ sɔrfʋ yuon ir nɩyɔɔ ka ba turo wʋ. Ba mɩ kʋ wʋ naa ka a bala jaa na turo wʋ mɩ bũbur.
44005038	A lɛ jũu, maa na 'yɛr yɩ naa ɩka yɩ ir nũu, tɩchɛ a nɩbɛ ba nyã bar. Yɩ bar ba a ba chiine. Ala ɩ a lɛ ban maala ɩn nɩrɛ lɛ bin an ɩn pɔrɔ.
44005039	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ lɛ a yi, yaa be jaa na wa tʋ̃ɔ ŋmaa a nɩbɛ banyãna sɔr ɛ, yɩn wa bɔ̃ɔn naa ka a ɩ Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ yɩ jɛɛrɛ nɩ."
44005040	A nɩbɛrɛ tu naa a lɛ a Gamaliel na 'yɛr, tɩ na ba bʋɔl a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ fɔb ba tɩ kpãkpãan ba ɩka ba taa lɛ ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr pʋrɔ nɩ a Yesu yuor go ɛ, tɩ bar ba a ba chen.
44005041	A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ na wa yi a nɩbɛrɛ banyãna niem, ba chɩlɛ naa, bojũu ba sɛɛn naa a dɔɔyɛ nɩ a vɩ̃ difʋ a Yesu yuor jũu.
44005042	Bɩbir jaa lɛ ba ma be a be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ wile a nɩbɛ na ba mɩ yʋɔrɔ a yie ba gala ɛ, na ba wile a nɩbɛ tɩ 'yɛrɛ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ ɩka a Yesu lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
44006001	A ber ala pɔ, a poturbo na waara pʋɔrɔ a bala ban dɔɔ a paal yuo pɔ, ka baa tʋɔrɔ 'yɛrɛ a Juu kɔkɔr ɛ, hũhũnõ na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bala na ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ, bojũu a ba pɔɔkɔɛ maa nyɛ a bɩbir jaa bʋ̃diir ban ma põ ɛ.
44006002	Be lɛ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ pie nɩ ayi bʋɔl a poturbo ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa wa 'yɛr, "A ba tara sɔr ka sɩn bar a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr 'yɛrfʋ tɩ põnõ bʋ̃diir ɛ.
44006003	A lɛ jũu yɛɛr, yɩ kaa a yɩ pɔ na yɩ ir dɔɔr ayopõi, bala yɩn bɔ̃ɔ ka ba sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ tɩ mɩ tara yɛ̃, ka sɩn de a tʋ̃mɔ̃ nyã kʋ ba.
44006004	Tɩchɛ a sɩn 'lɔ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ nɩ a wʋ 'yɛr."
44006005	A 'yɛr nyã pɛl ba jaa na duo a be pʋɔ, ka ba ir a nɩbɛ banyãna. Sɩteven a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na sɛɛ ka wʋ mɩ tara sɔɔfʋ, nɩ Filip, nɩ Porokorusɩ, nɩ Nɩkanor, nɩ Tɩmon, nɩ Pamenasɩ, nɩ Nikolasɩ na yi Antiok na wʋ lɩɛb kpɛ a Juu nɩbɛ puorfʋ pɔ.
44006006	A nɩbɛ banyãna lɛ ba ir waan a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ sɛ̃, ka ba dɔɔl ba nuur sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ba.
44006007	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr yaar, ka a poturbo mɩ na be a Jerusalɛm pʋɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃. A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlorbo yɔɔ jie mɩ sɔɔn de a 'yɛr.
44006008	Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ ben a Sɩteven sɛ̃ ka wʋ tara kpɛ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃yɔɔ a nɩbɛ sɛ̃.
44006009	A nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie a ba bʋɔl ba, Mɩ̃ɛ Sorbo, nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi a Sirenɩ nɩ a Aleksandiriya, ka bamɩne mɩ yi a Sɩlɩsɩya nɩ Asɩya. A nɩbɛ banyãna lɛ piel a nɛchɩrɛ na ba chɩrɛ nɩ a Sɩteven.
44006010	Tɩchɛ baa tʋɔrɔ wʋ ɛ, a yɛ̃ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na kʋ wʋ a wʋ 'yɛrɛ nɩ.
44006011	A ba pãa sɔɔl tʋ̃ nɩbɛ bamɩne ka ba ŋmaa jir 'yɛr ɩka, "Sɩn lɛ wõ a Sɩteven na fere 'yɛrɛ 'yɛrdɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Mosesɩ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn."
44006012	Tɩ tɔ a nɩbɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe 'yɔ̃ɔ ka ba nyɔɔ a Sɩteven chiin a ba 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ sɛ̃.
44006013	Be lɛ ba waan jir ŋmarba ka ba wa 'yɛr, "A daba nyãna ba gala 'yɛr dɛbɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir chɛchɛ nyãna ɛ, nɩ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wʋn bin ɛ.
44006014	Sɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ wõ wʋn 'yɛr ɩka a Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ na ŋmɛr a jie nyãna, tɩ na wʋ lɩɛb a binfʋ ala a Mosesɩ na dɔ̃ɔ bin kʋ sɩ."
44006015	Ka a bala jaa na jɩ̃nɛ a be a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie, kãan a Sɩteven nie ka wʋ kaara fɩka a malaka nie.
44007001	Be lɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sʋʋr wʋ, "Sɩrɛ lɛ a anyãna ban 'yɛr bɩɩ?"
44007002	Ka a Sɩteven haa 'yɛr, "Yɛɛr nɩ sãamɩne, yɩ chɛlɛ. A Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr sʋɔ dɔ̃ɔ yi a sɩ sãa Abraham lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ chɛnɛ be a Mesopotamiya wɛr pɔ sɛrɛ tɩ wa chen a Haran.
44007003	A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'Yi a fʋ tẽe na fʋ bar a fʋ nɩbɛ tɩ na fʋ chen wɛr yuo pɔ ɩn na wiil fʋ.'
44007004	"A wʋ yi a Chaldea wɛr pɔ na wʋ chen tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a Haran wɛr pɔ. A wʋ sãa na wa kpi baar lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn waan wʋ a kana yɩn ben kpɩɛrɛ.
44007005	Nãaŋmɩn ba kʋ wʋ bon jaa a kana ɛ, waa kʋ wʋ jibile jaa gba ɛ, bɩɩ gbɛr nɛfʋ jie ɛ. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn tɩr nɛɛ kʋ wʋ ɩka 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ yɔn lɛ na so a jie, tɩ waa tara bie gba ɛ.
44007006	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ a Abraham, 'A fʋ yɔn na ɩ naa sãanba paal sãan pɔ, na ba ɩ gbãgbaar ka ba ge ba yuom kɔɔr anaar (400).
44007007	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa, ɩka wʋn yaa naa a sãn a paal 'lɔ na maal ba a gbãgbaar. A anyã puor lɛ ban wa puor ma a jie nyãna.'
44007008	Nãaŋmɩn tɩr nɛɛ kʋ a Abraham a yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ yele. Abraham na wa dɔɔ a Isaakɩ, wʋ ŋmaa wʋn a yʋɔr a ber aniin daar. Ka a Isaakɩ mɩ dɔɔ a Jekɔb, ka a Jekɔb mɩ dɔɔ a sɩ sãamɩne pie nɩ ayi.
44007009	"A sɩ sãamɩne banyãna na tara nɩ a ba yɛbile Josefʋ nɩ nyuur jũu, na ba nyɔɔ wʋ da kʋ a Ijipitɩ dẽme. Tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn be a wʋ sɛ̃.
44007010	Na wʋ faa wʋ yin a wʋ wõm a jaa pɔ. Wʋ kʋ naa a Josefʋ yɛ̃ na wʋ sʋ̃ʋ wʋ a wʋ nyɛ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ a Faaro na ɩ a Ijipitɩ nãa niem, na wʋ maal wʋ ka wʋ ɩ a Ijipitɩ nɩ a nãa jie wʋ jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ.
44007011	"Ka a kɔ̃ lo Ijipitɩ nɩ a Kanaan wɛr wʋ jaa waan dɔɔyɛ, ka a sɩ sãamɩne ba nyɛrɛ bʋ̃diir ɛ.
44007012	Jekɔb na wa wõ ɩka bʋ̃diir ben a be Ijipitɩ, wʋ tʋ̃n a sɩ sãamɩne ka ba chen.
44007013	A gbɛɛ ayi sʋɔ ban chen lɛ a Josefʋ wiil a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ ba, ka a Faaro mɩ pãa bɔ̃ɔ a Josefʋ yir nɩbɛ.
44007014	A anyã puor lɛ a Josefʋ tʋ̃ bʋɔl a wʋ sãa Jekɔb nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme, a ba jaa ɩ nɩbɛ lɩjaata nɩ pie nɩ anũu (75).
44007015	Jekɔb chen a be a Ijipitɩ nɩ a sɩ sãamɩne be lɛ ba jaa tɩ kpi.
44007016	Ba tuo naa a ba ɩ̃gãma waan a Sekem wa ũu ba a yaa 'lɔ pɔ a Abraham na da a Hamor bibiir sɛ̃ a be a Sekem.
44007017	"A sɔ̃ɔ na wa gbʋr ka a Nãaŋmɩn na maal a lɛ wʋn tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a Abraham, a sɩ nɩbɛ na be a Ijipitɩ dɔɔn paal.
44007018	Ala lɛ ka a nãyuo wa di na wʋ kaara a Ijipitɩ na waa bɔ̃ɔ a Josefʋ yele ɛ.
44007019	Wʋ maal naa a sɩ nɩbɛ putuyele na wʋ ge ba, na wʋ ma fɩr a pɔɔ pʋʋr ka bala wa dɔɔ bipɩlɛ ba lɔb ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ a ba kpi.
44007020	"A sɔ̃ɔ nyãna lɛ ba dɔɔ a Mosesɩ, ka wʋ ɩ bivɩla a Nãaŋmɩn niem. A ba guol wʋ ŋmɛrsɩ ata be a wʋ sãa yir.
44007021	Ban wa yin wʋ tɩ bar a yõo, Faaro bipɔɔ de wʋn guol ka wʋ ɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ bidaba.
44007022	Ba jãn naa Mosesɩ a Ijipitɩ tẽe yɛ̃ a jaa, ka wʋ kpɛ̃mɛ a wʋ 'yɛr nɩ a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ.
44007023	"A lɛ a Mosesɩ na wa ta yuom lɩjaayi (40), wʋ tɩɛr naa a wʋ yɛɛr Isɩral nɩbɛ na wʋ ɩka wʋ chen tɩ piir ba kaa.
44007024	Wʋ tɩ nyɛn a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ a Ijipitɩ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na gere ka wʋ ŋmaa de na wʋ kʋ a Ijipitɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ.
44007025	Mosesɩ tɩɛr lɛ ɩka a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ na bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka 'lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na de faan ba, tɩchɛ baa tɩɛrtɔ a lɛ ɛ.
44007026	A wɛr na wa chaar, wʋ tɩ nyɛn a Isɩral nɩbɛ ayi mɩ na jɛɛrɛ taa. Ka wʋ 'maal ba tɩ sʋrɔ ba, 'Yɩn yɛɛr nara, bo lɛ so a yɩ jɛɛrɛ taa?'
44007027	Tɩchɛ a 'lɔ sʋɔ na tʋ̃ɔ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ daan a Mosesɩ bar tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, 'An tʋ̃ fʋ ɩka fʋ wa kaara sɩ na fʋ tɔɔrɔ a sɩ 'yɛr?
44007028	Fʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka fʋ mɩ kʋ ma nɩtãa lɛ fʋn kʋ a Ijipitɩ nɩrɛ a jãa wɛ?'
44007029	Mosesɩ na wõ a 'yɛr nyãna ka wʋ jo chen tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a Midiyan, be lɛ wʋ be na wʋ wa dɔɔ dabil ayi.
44007030	"Yuom lɩjaayi (40) na wa po, malaka wa lɩɛb bũu lɩrɛ tɩbile pɔ, na wʋ dũu a Mosesɩ be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ na gbʋr a Sinai tɔ̃ɔ par.
44007031	Wʋn wa nyɛ a lɛ ka a nɛ'maa wʋ, a wʋ tɔɔ gbʋr ɩka wʋ kaa. Be lɛ wʋ wõ a Soro kɔkɔr na 'yɛr,
44007032	''Maa lɛ ɩ a fʋ sãamɩne Nãaŋmɩn, Abraham, Isaakɩ nɩ a Jekɔb Nãaŋmɩn.' Ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a Mosesɩ waa lɛ 'lara na kaa ɛ.
44007033	"Ka a sɩ Soro pãa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, 'Yaa a fʋ nafɔɔr bar, a jie fʋn ara ɩ naa jichɛchɛ.
44007034	N nyɛ naa a n nɩbɛ be a Ijipitɩ pɔ ban gere, n wõ naa ba hʋ̃ʋnfʋ naa suu ɩka n wa faa ba. Wa, ka n tʋ̃ fʋ a be a Ijipitɩ.'
44007035	"A Mosesɩ nyãna nɩ wʋ ju ban tɔr bar tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, 'An lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ ɩka fʋ kaara sɩ na fʋ tɔɔrɔ a sɩ 'yɛr?' 'Lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ tʋ̃ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a malaka na wa dũu wʋ 'lɩrɛ a bũu a tɩbile pɔ, ɩka wʋ tɩ ɩ a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a ba fafaara.
44007036	'Lɔ lɛ tɩ de ba nie na wʋ tʋ̃ tʋ̃ yɔɔ be a Ijipitɩ tẽe pɔ, nɩ a Man Jɩɛ par nɩ a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ ban be a yuom lɩjaayi (40).
44007037	A Mosesɩ nyãna nɩ wʋ ju lɛ 'yɛr kʋ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ɩka, 'Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ naa a 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ a maa kaar ka wʋ yi a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ pɔ.'
44007038	Wʋ dɔ̃ɔ pʋɔ a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ, 'matãan a sɩ sãakpãmɩne ka a malaka 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ wʋ be a Sinai Tɔ̃ɔ par na ɩ nyɛvʋr 'yɛr ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ sɩ.
44007039	"Tɩchɛ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne tɔr wʋ naa, na baa tu a wʋ nɛɛ ɛ. Ba tɔr wʋn bar ka a ba tɩɛr lɩɛb chen be a Ijipitɩ.
44007040	Ba 'yɛr kʋ a Aaron, 'Maal ŋmɩmɛ kʋ sɩ ka a ma de sɩ nie, a Mosesɩ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na yin sɩ a Ijipitɩ saa bɔ̃ɔ bo nɩ tara wʋ ɛ.'
44007041	A ba mɛ bʋtɩɩ a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ka wʋ nyɛtãan nele, na ba waan bomo wa lon bɔɔr a jie na ba dɩ̃ɛn 'yɔ̃ɔn a ba nũu bʋ̃maalaa nyãna.
44007042	Tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ ba, na wʋ bar ba ka ba puoro a saaju bomo. Ka anyãna tɩ tuor a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb, wʋ sʋʋr naa, 'A yɩn Isɩral nɩbɛ, yɩn be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ a yuom lɩjaayi (40) na yɩ dɔ̃ɔ waan a bɔɔrlo bomo maa lɛ yɩ wa kʋ bɩɩ?
44007043	Kai, tɩ a bʋtɩbɛ ala yɩn kaara lɛ a Molokɩ nɩ ŋmɛrbir ŋmɩn Arefan, a tɩbɛ anyãna lɛ yɩ dɔ̃ɔ maal puoro. A lɛ jũu, ɩn vɛ̃ naa ka ba nyɔɔr yɩ chiin a Babilon puor ka yɩ tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a be.'
44007044	"A sɩ sãakpãmɩne dɔ̃ɔ maal gãma yir be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ ka a ɩ dãasɩɛ, ba maal wʋ naa nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na man wiil a Mosesɩ ka wʋ nyɛ.
44007045	A gãma yir nyã lɛ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne tara ka a Josua de ba a nie ka ba waan, a ba wa faa a wɛr nyã pɔ a nɩyor na dɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn dii ba bar. A gãn yir nyã ben be lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ tãn a Nãa David sɔ̃ɔ.
44007046	Nãaŋmɩn maal vɩla kʋ wʋ ka wʋ ɩka wʋn mɛn yir kʋ a Jekɔb Nãaŋmɩn.
44007047	Tɩchɛ Solomon lɛ wa mɛ a yir kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn.
44007048	"Fʋ̃ʋ kaa, a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ a saaju sʋɔ, ba kpɩɛrɛ a yie anyã nɩbɛ na mɛ ɛ. Nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr,
44007049	'Saaju lɛ ɩ a maa nakɔɔ, ka a tẽe ɩ a n gbɛɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie. Ka a sɩ Soro sʋʋr, yir bo tɔ lɛ yɩn mɛ kʋ ma? Bɩɩ nyɩnɛ lɛ na ɩ a n pɛ̃nfʋ jie?
44007050	A ba ɩ a maa nũu lɛ maal anyãna a jaa ɛ?'
44007051	"Yɩn nyãkpɩ̃ɛn dẽme na ɩ nɩbɛ na ba wõnõ 'yɛr ɛ, yɩ kaara a yɩ sãamɩne kaar. Yɩ maa sɔɔ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɔr ɛ.
44007052	Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ jaa ba be be ka a yɩ sãamɩne ba ge wʋ ɛ. Ba gba kʋ naa bala na de nie mʋɔl 'yɛr a Torfʋ Sʋɔ 'lɔ waa 'yɛr. A pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩn gba lɛ gar 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ na yɩ kʋ wʋ.
44007053	Yɩn lɛ de a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ wʋn kʋ a malaka a wʋ wa kʋ yɩ ka yɩ de tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ, tɩchɛ a yɩ tɔr bar."
44007054	A 'yɛr nyãna ban wa wõ, ka ba suur ir a ba kpar kparaa jur 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ.
44007055	Tɩchɛ a Sɩteven a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na sɛɛ a wʋ dʋl kaa saaju na wʋ nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr, ka a Yesu ara a Nãaŋmɩn nũsʋ̃ɔ jie.
44007056	Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Yɩ nyɛ ka, n nyɛ naa saaju na yuo ka a Nɩsaal Bie ara a Nãaŋmɩn nũsʋ̃ɔ jie."
44007057	A anyãna ban wõ ba pɔɔn a tobo tɩ ŋme chɛlma na ba tɩ mɩl wʋ,
44007058	na ba tɔɔ wʋ yin a tẽe chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ tɩ piel lɔɔrɔ wʋ nɩ kʋsɩbɛ. Ka a bala na di dãasɩɛ yaar a ba fuusɩ bin pɔlbile kɔ̃ɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Sɔɔl sɛ̃.
44007059	Ban lɔɔrɔ wʋ a lɛ nɛ na kʋ ka wʋ sʋɔr Yesu, "N Soro Yesu de a n sɩ̃ɛ."
44007060	Wʋ lon gbur dumo tɩ pãa ŋme chɛlma 'yɛr, "N Soro taa ɩrɛ wa yaara ba sãn ɛ." A anyãna lɛ wʋ 'yɛr baar tɩ ŋmaa vʋʋr.
44008001	A Sɔɔl mɩ dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ ɩka ba kʋ a Sɩteven. A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ jaa lɛ ba piel gere a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo be a Jerusalɛm. Ka ba jaa ŋma yaar a bamɩne chen Judiya a bamɩne mɩ chen Samariya tɩchɛ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ tɛɛ be a Jerusalɛm.
44008002	Nɩbɛ bamɩne na joro a Nãaŋmɩn 'mɔɔn a Sɩteven ũu tɩ na ba kõ a kuor.
44008003	Tɩchɛ ka a Sɔɔl mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir bur buro a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ bara, na wʋ yʋɔrɔ kpɩɛrɛ a yie nyɔɔrɔ dɔɔr nɩ pɔbɔ tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ.
44008004	A bala na jo ŋma a dẽdẽme chɛnɛ na mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr jie jaa ban chen.
44008005	Filip chen Samariya tẽe pɔ, na wʋ tɩ 'yɛr ɩka Yesu lɛ a Nɩ-iraa a be.
44008006	A nɩyɔɔ na wa wõ a lɛ a Filip na 'yɛr tɩ mɩ nyɛ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ wʋn tʋ̃, a ba yuo toor chɛlɛ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ.
44008007	A sɩdɛbɛ ala na dɔ̃ɔ pɔɔrɔ a nɩbɛ ŋmen chɛlsɩ wa yin a nɩbɛ pɔ, ka a gbɛkũn nɩ a gbɛrsɩ yɔɔ jaa sa.
44008008	Ka a tẽe 'lɔ dẽme ba jaa chɩlɛ.
44008009	Daba kɔ̃ɔ dɔ̃ɔ be be ban bʋɔlɔ Simon na wʋ ma tʋ̃nɔ̃ tɩ̃sɔɔ tʋ̃mɔ̃ ka a 'maa a Samariya nɩbɛ nɛɛ, na wʋ ma wile a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɩka nɩkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ.
44008010	A nɩbɛ ba jaa, a bɛrɛ nɩ a bil ba jaa ma yuon toor chɛlɛ wʋ tɩ 'yɛrɛ, "A daba nyã 'lɔ kpɛ̃ɔ ɩ naa a gãdaa sʋɔ kpɛ̃ɔ."
44008011	Ba turo wʋ naa bojũu a kor naa wʋn tʋ̃nɔ̃ a tɩ̃sɔɔ tʋ̃mɔ̃ ka a 'maa ba nɛɛ.
44008012	Tɩchɛ a lɛ ban wa sɔɔ de a lɛ a Filip na 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr, nɩ a Yesu na ɩ a Nɩ-iraa yuor, dɔɔr nɩ pɔbɔ ba jaa son a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
44008013	A Simon mɩ sɔɔ naa ka ba so wʋ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ a wʋ turo a Filip yʋɔrɔ, a nɛ'maa tʋ̃yɔɔ wʋn nyɛ wʋn tʋ̃.
44008014	A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ na be a Jerusalɛm na wa wõ ɩka a Samariya nɩbɛ mɩ sɔɔn de a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr, ba tʋ̃n Pita nɩ Jɔɔn a ba sɛ̃.
44008015	Ban tɩ ta, ba sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ a nɩbɛ ka ban nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ.
44008016	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ba kpɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa sɛrɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ lɛ ba so ba, nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor.
44008017	Ka a Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn pãa dɔɔl ba a nuur a ba nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ.
44008018	Simon na nyɛ a lɛ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ na dɔɔl ba a nũu ka ba nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ, a wʋ de libie kʋ ba,
44008019	tɩ 'yɛr, "Yɩ mɩ kʋ ma a kpɛ̃ɔ nyãna ka maa wa dɔɔl nɩrɛ jaa a n nũu, a wʋ mɩ ma nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ."
44008020	Ka a Pita 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a fʋ libie jaa yɩ wɛ, bojũu fʋ tɩɛr ɩka fʋn tʋ̃ɔ da a Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ nɩ libie.
44008021	Faa tara sɔr na lɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃n sɩ ɛ, bojũu a fʋ nyãa ba tor a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ.
44008022	Lɩɛb a fʋ pututɩɛr nyãna na fʋ sʋɔr a sɩ Soro amɩne sɛ̃ wʋn vɛ̃n kʋ fʋ a fʋ tɩɛr dɛɛr nyãna fʋn tara.
44008023	N nyɛn bɔ̃ɔn fʋn ɩ pubier sʋɔ ka a yelbier nyɔɔ fʋ pɔɔ."
44008024	A Simon pãa 'yɛr, "Yɩ sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ma ka ala yɩn 'yɛr taa waara a n sɛ̃ ɛ."
44008025	A lɛ Pita nɩ a Jɔɔn na wa man 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr baar, ba lɩɛb kulo a Jerusalɛm ba 'yɛrɛ naa a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna a tẽbil ala na chɛɛl a Samariya.
44008026	Nãaŋmɩn malaka 'yɛr kʋ a Filip, "Ir suu de a sɔr 'lɔ na yi a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ tu a Jerusalɛm chen a Gaja."
44008027	Lɛ lɛ wʋ ir chiine, na wʋ tɩ tuor a Etiyopiya daba ɩ̃sʋɔ ban maal ka wʋ ab na wʋ ɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kaara a Etiyopiya nãpɔɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Kandasɩ libie. Jerusalɛm lɛ wʋ chen tɩ puor,
44008028	na wʋ lɩɛb kulo jɩ̃nɛ a wʋ wii torko pɔ na wʋ kara a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Isaiya gãn.
44008029	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr a Filip, "Chen tɩ gbʋr a torko par."
44008030	A Filip jo chen a be a torko par na wʋ wõ a daba na kara a Isaiya gãn a wʋ sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa lɛ par fʋn kara ɔ?"
44008031	Ka a daba 'yɛr, "Ŋmɩnɛ ɩn ɩrɛ wa bɔ̃ɔ a par, ka nɩrɛ baa wiil ma ɛ?" Tɩ na wʋ bʋɔl a Filip ka wʋ do jɩ̃nɛ a torko pɔ.
44008032	A anyãna lɛ a da-abbaa 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ dɔ̃ɔ kara a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Ba nyɔɔ wʋn chiine fɩka pɛr na tɩ kʋ, Wʋ ɩn jaa gbul fɩka pele ban põnõ a kɔɔl na waa haa nɛɛ ɛ.
44008033	Wʋ siir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a lɛ ban ba tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr kaa tor ɛ. An lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr a wʋ bal nɩbɛ 'yɛr? A wʋ nyɛvʋr ba tal tɛɛr a ka a wɛr pɔ ɛ."
44008034	Ka a da-abbaa nyã sʋɔr a Filip, "Yãayãabɩlɛ, 'yɛr kʋ ma, an 'yɛr lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ nyã 'yɛrɛ? Wʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ bɩɩ nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ?"
44008035	A Filip pãa piel na wʋ de a Nãaŋmɩn gãn 'yɛr nyãna man a Yesu 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ wʋ.
44008036	Ban 'mataa chiine tɩ ta kʋ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ par a sɔr pɔ, ka a da-abbaa 'lɔ 'yɛr, "Nyɛ kʋ̃ɔ, bãa lɛ so ka fʋ kʋ̃ so ma a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ɛ?"
44008038	Tɩ na wʋ tɔɔ a torko a wʋ ara, ka a 'lɔ nɩ a Filip 'mataa kpɛ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ, ka a Filip so wʋ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
44008039	Ban wa yi a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ, Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wa jaa naa a Filip chiin ka a da-abbaa 'lɔ ba lɛ nyɛ wʋ go ɛ. Tɩ de wʋ sɔr chɩlɛ kulo.
44008040	Tɩchɛ ka a Filip tɩ yi naa Ajotusɩ na wʋ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr a tẽn ala a jaa tɩ tãn Sisariya.
44009001	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a Sɔɔl chɛnɛ pʋrɔ a sɩ Soro poturbo ju, na wʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ kʋ ba. Wʋ chen naa a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sɛ̃,
44009002	na wʋ tɩ sʋɔr sɔr de gãn na chiin a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir ala na be a Damaskus ɩka 'lɔ wa tɩ nyɛ nɩrɛ na turo a Sɔr nyã, ka pɔɔ lɛ bɩɩ daba lɛ wʋ tʋ̃ɔ nyɔɔr ba waan a Jerusalɛm.
44009003	Ala lɛ wʋ de a sɔr chiine tɩ gbʋrɔ a Damaskus ka chãa yi be a saaju ajienaa wa nyɩɩr jil wʋ.
44009004	Ka wʋ lo tẽe tɩ wõ kɔkɔr na bʋɔlɔ wʋ sʋrɔ, "Sɔɔl, Sɔɔl, bo lɛ so a fʋ gere ma a lɛ?"
44009005	Ka a Sɔɔl sʋʋr, "An lɛ fʋ ɩ Soro?" Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ ɩ a Yesu fʋn gere.
44009006	Pʋ̃pãanyã, ir na fʋ kpɛ be a tẽe pɔ, ban wiil fʋ naa a lɛ fʋn na ɩ."
44009007	Ka a dɔɔr bala nɩ a Sɔɔl na 'mataa chiine gĩe ara, na ba wõ a dɔɔn, tɩchɛ baa nyɛ nɩrɛ ɛ.
44009008	Ka a Sɔɔl ir a tẽe ara na wʋ yuo a nɩbie tɩ waa lɛ nyɛrɛ ɛ. A ba nyɔɔ wʋ a nũu tɔɔ kpɛ̃n be a Damaskus.
44009009	Wʋ maal ber ata waa lɛ nyɛrɛ ɛ, waa di bʋ̃diir bɩɩ nyũ kʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
44009010	Tɩchɛ a poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ben a be Damaskus a ba bʋɔlɔ wʋ Ananias ka a sɩ Soro wa bʋɔl wʋ a jãna pɔ, "Ananias." A wʋ sɔɔ, "Ɔ̃ɔ, n Soro."
44009011	Ka a Soro 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Ir de a Sɔr Dẽdẽe chiine na fʋ tɩ ta a Judas yir sʋʋr daba na yi Tasusɩ a ba bʋɔlɔ Sɔɔl, be lɛ wʋ be sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn.
44009012	A wʋ jãna pɔ, wʋ nyɛn daba ban bʋɔlɔ Ananias na dɔɔl wʋ nũu ka wʋ lɛ nyɛrɛ."
44009013	A Ananias 'yɛr, "N Soro, n wõn a daba nyã yelyɔɔ a lɛ wʋn ge a fʋ nɩsʋ̃n a be a Jerusalɛm.
44009014	A ka mɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ mɩ kʋ wʋn sɔr ɩka wʋ wa nyɔɔr a bala jaa na bʋɔlɔ a fʋ yuor."
44009015	Tɩchɛ ka a Soro 'yɛr kʋ a Ananias, "Chen, a daba nyãna lɛ ɩ a n bʋ̃-iraa ka wʋn tuo a maa yuor chiin a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ pɔ, nɩ a ba nãmɩne sɛ̃, lɔ̃ɔn a Isɩral nɩbɛ.
44009016	Ɩ̃n wiil wʋ naa a lɛ wʋn na di dɔɔyɛ a n yuor jũu."
44009017	Be lɛ a Ananias ir chen tɩ kpɛ be a yir, na wʋ tɩ dɔɔl wʋ a nũu tɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "N yɛbɛ Sɔɔl, a sɩ Soro Yesu na yi fʋ be a sɔr pɔ fʋn waara lɛ tʋ̃ ma a fʋ sɛ̃ ka fʋn lɛ nyɛrɛ go, na fʋ sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ."
44009018	Ajienaa ka bʋ̃nyɩnsɩ 'lɔɔr a Sɔɔl nɩbie pɔ lo a wʋ lɛ nyɛrɛ go. Wʋ ir naa a ba tɔ̃ɔ so wʋ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
44009019	Wʋn wa di a bʋ̃diir baar wʋ lɛ nyɛn kpɛ̃ɔ, na wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a poturbo bala sɛ̃ a be a Damaskus bɩ̃lãa.
44009020	Ajienaa, wʋ piel 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr be a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir, na wʋ 'yɛrɛ ɩka a Yesu ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn Bie.
44009021	Bala jaa na wõ a wʋ 'yɛr ka a 'maa ba nɛɛ a ba sʋrɔ, "A ba ɩ a daba nyãna lɛ ir gere a bala a be a Jerusalɛm na bʋɔlɔ a yuor nyãna ɛ? Na wʋ wa a ka mɩ ɩka wʋ wa nyɔɔr a bala mɩ chiin tɩ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ ɛ?"
44009022	Tɩchɛ ka a Sɔɔl kpɛ̃ɔ chɛnɛ pʋɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ka wʋ 'yɛr tʋ̃ɔ a Juu nɩbɛ na kpɩɛrɛ a Damaskus na wʋ wiil ba ɩka a Yesu lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
44009023	Ber yɔɔ na wa po, a Juu nɩbɛ guor taa ɩka ba kʋ a Sɔɔl,
44009024	tɩchɛ kaa a Sɔɔl bɔ̃ɔn a ba guorfʋ. Mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ jaa lɛ ba mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir guro wʋ a tẽe dɔ̃dɔɩ nɛɛr, bʋɔrɔ a wʋ kʋ̃ fʋ.
44009025	Tɩchɛ ka a bala na turo wʋ 'mɔɔ wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ pɩɛ pɔ tɩ̃sɔɔ na ba tur wʋ bar ka wʋ tu a dãpuor dachin pɔ suu.
44009026	Wʋn tɩ ta Jerusalɛm, wʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a poturbo tɩchɛ a ba joro wʋ dãbɩ̃ɛ, baa sɔɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ naa a poturo ɩ̃sʋɔ ɛ.
44009027	Tɩchɛ ka a Banabasɩ tara wʋ chiin be a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ sɛ̃. 'Lɔ lɛ pãa man kʋ ba a lɛ a Sɔɔl na nyɛ a sɩ Soro a sɔr pɔ, ka a Soro 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ wʋ. Wʋ 'yɛr ɩka a be a Damaskus wʋ mʋɔl 'yɛr a Yesu yuor 'yɛr, na wʋ ta jo dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
44009028	A Sɔɔl jɩ̃nɛ a be a ba sɛ̃ na wʋ so wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yʋɔrɔ be a Jerusalɛm na wʋ mʋɔlɔ a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor 'yɛrɛ ba joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
44009029	Wʋ ma 'yɛrɛ naa ka a 'lɔ nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bala ban dɔɔ a paal yuo pɔ ka baa tʋɔrɔ 'yɛrɛ a Juu kɔkɔr ɛ, ma chɩrɛ taa, ka ba bʋɔrɔ a wʋ kʋfʋ.
44009030	A poturbo na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃ ba tara wʋn chiin a Sisariya tɩ bar ka wʋ chen Tasusɩ.
44009031	Damfʋ ba lɛ be a bala na puoro be a Judiya, Galilee nɩ a Samariya, ka a nyã'maar. Ba kpɛ̃mɛ naa ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ ka ba nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ na ba joro a sɩ Soro dãbɩ̃ɛ.
44009032	Ka a Pita yʋɔrɔ a tẽn na wʋ wa chen Lida ɩka wʋ tɩ piir a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo kaa.
44009033	Be lɛ wʋ tɩ nyɛ daba ban bʋɔlɔ Ainɩyas na gbɛr gã yuomo aniin.
44009034	Ka a Pita bʋɔl wʋ, "Ainɩyas, Yesu yuor pɔ, sa. Ir saaju na fʋ pilʋ̃ a fʋ bʋ̃gãnaa." Ajienaa lɛ a Ainɩyas ir saaju.
44009035	Ka a Lida nɩbɛ ba jaa nɩ a Saron nɩbɛ na nyɛ a lɛ, a ba lɩɛb puoro a sɩ Soro.
44009036	Pɔɔ kɔ̃ɔ mɩ na dɔ̃ɔ puoro ben a be Jopa, ka ba bʋɔlɔ wʋ Tabita, a yo bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ba lɩɛb bʋɔlɔ Dɔɔkas. Wʋ ma maala na vɩla na wʋ sʋ̃nɔ̃ a nɔ̃n dẽme.
44009037	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ wʋ ɩ baal na wʋ kpi, a ba so wʋ a kʋ̃ɔ don gaal be a bɔɔpɩɛ pɔ.
44009038	Lida nɩ a Jopa mɩ ba jãa ɛ, kaa a pupuorbo wõ ɩka a Pita ben a Lida, a ba tʋ̃ nɩbɛ ayi ka ba tɩ sʋɔr wʋ, "Yãayãabɩlɛ a wʋ wa fɔɔ."
44009039	Ka bala naa Pita jaa 'mataa chen, wʋn wa ta ba de wʋn don be a bɔɔpɩɛ die pɔ. A pɔɔkɔɛ ba jaa ara na jilʋ̃ wʋ kõnõ na ba wile a Pita a fuusɩ nɩ a fɔɔr a Dɔɔkas na maal wʋn dɔ̃ɔ chɛnɛ be a ba sɛ̃.
44009040	Pita diin ba jaa a ba yi a be a die pɔ, tɩ na wʋ gbur dumo sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn, na wʋ lɩɛb tor a kũu tɩ 'yɛr, "Tabita ir." A wʋ yuo a nɩbie nyɛ a Pita na wʋ ir jɩ̃nɛ.
44009041	Ka a Pita nyɔɔ wʋ a nũu sʋ̃ʋ wʋ a wʋ ir ara, tɩ pãa bʋɔl a bala na sɔɔ nɩ a pɔɔkɔɛ ka ba kpɛ wa nyɛ a wʋ ɩ nɩ nɩbir.
44009042	Ka a yele nyãna yaar a Jopa wʋ jaa ka a nɩbɛ yɔɔ jie wa sɔɔ a sɩ Soro.
44009043	A Pita jɛ̃n be a Jopa bɩ̃lãa a daba kɔ̃ɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Simon na ma nɔ̃nɔ̃ gãma yir.
44010001	Be a Sisariya, daba kɔ̃ɔ dɔ̃ɔ be be a ba bʋɔlɔ wʋ Konɩlɩyɔs, wʋ be naa a sojasɩ gbul 'lɔ pɔ a Itali nɩbɛ na bʋɔlɔ a sojasɩ kɔbaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ.
44010002	'Lɔ naa wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa puoro naa na ba joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ, na wʋ ma kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ bala an wõnõ pɔrɔ, na wʋ mɩ ma sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn ba gala ɛ.
44010003	Bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wa bal, a wʋ gã jãn jaa chɛchɛ nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn malaka a wʋ wa ara a wʋ sɛ̃ tɩ bʋɔl wʋ, "Konɩlɩyɔs."
44010004	Ka wʋ chaal a lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ tɩ sʋʋr, "Bo lɛ N Soro?" Ka a malaka 'yɛr, "A fʋ puorfʋ nɩ a kʋfʋ fʋn kʋrɔ a nɔ̃n dẽme don tɩ pɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn ka wʋ tara a fʋ tɩɛr.
44010005	Pʋ̃pãanyã, tʋ̃ nɩbɛ ka ba chen a Jopa tɩ tara daba kɔ̃ɔ na di Simon tɩ ba bʋɔlɔ wʋ Pita a wʋ wa.
44010006	Wʋ kpɩɛrɛ naa a daba na nɔ̃nɔ̃ gãma mɩ na di a Simon yir, ka a wʋ yir gbʋr a man kpɛ̃ɛ gogoro."
44010007	A malaka na wa chen baar, Konɩlɩyɔs bʋɔl naa a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ayi nɩ a soja ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ na puoro na ma sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ.
44010008	Wʋ man a lɛ jaa na ɩ tɩ tʋ̃ ba a Jopa.
44010009	A wɛr na wa chaar mɔ̃tɔ̃tuo sʋ̃ɔ, ka ba be a sɔr pɔ chiine tɩ gbʋrɔ a tẽe, a Pita mɩ don a gar ju Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jie.
44010010	Ka a kɔ̃ kpɛ wʋ a wʋ bʋɔrɔ bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ na di, ban chɛnɛ maala a bʋ̃diir ka a dedee kpɛ wʋ.
44010011	A wʋ nyɛ saaju na yuo a wʋ nyɛ bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ fɩka fɔkpɛ̃ɛ na gbũ jiir anaar ka wʋ suro wa gbʋrɔ a tẽe.
44010012	Ka a dʋ̃gbɛɛ anaar a jaa bʋrɔ be be nɩ a tẽe bʋ̃vʋʋrsɩ nɩ a lubilɔɔrsɩ a jaa.
44010013	Be lɛ a kɔkɔr pãa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Pita, ir kʋ 'wɔb."
44010014	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita 'yɛr, "Sɩrɛ jaa, kai. N Soro, n ba 'wɔb a dʋ̃dɛbɛ anyãna nɩ a dʋ̃chiirsɩ anyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ɛ."
44010015	Ka a kɔkɔr lɛ 'yɛr go, "Ta bʋɔl bon jaa bʋ̃dɛɛr 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na maal a wʋ ɩ bʋ̃sʋ̃ ɛ."
44010016	Gbɛɛ ata lɛ a ɩ, tɩchɛ ka a fɔbaa lɛ jaa a lɛ nɛ don a saaju ajienaa.
44010017	Lɛ a Pita na chɛnɛ pɛrɛ a nyɛfʋ nyã par, ka a dɔɔr bala a Konɩlɩyɔs na tʋ̃ mɩ nyɛn a Simon yir na ba ara a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ.
44010018	Ba bʋɔl sʋʋr, "Daba na di Simon tɩ ba bʋɔlɔ wʋ Pita ka lɛ wʋ kpɩɛrɛ ɔ?"
44010019	Lɛ a Pita na chɛnɛ tɩɛrɛ a nyɛfʋ nyãna ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Simon, dɔɔr ata lɛ bʋɔrɔ fʋ sʋrɔ.
44010020	Ir suu a ba sɛ̃, taa ɩrɛ wa baala fʋn na lɔ̃ɔ chiin ba ɛ, maa lɛ tʋ̃ ba."
44010021	Ka a Pita ir suu tɩ nyɛ a nɩbɛ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ ɩ a nɩrɛ yɩn bʋɔrɔ, bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ wa?"
44010022	A ba 'yɛr, "Konɩlɩyɔs na ɩ a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sɛ̃ lɛ sɩ yi. A wʋ yele tor naa ka wʋ ɩ nɩrɛ na joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ ba jaa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ. A Nãaŋmɩn malaka wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ɩka wʋ bʋɔl fʋ a fʋ wa be a wʋ yir a wʋ wõ lɛ jaa fʋn na man."
44010023	A Pita pãa tara ba kpɛ̃n tɩ gaal. Ka a wɛr chaar, a bala nɩ a Pita nɩ a pupuorbiir bamɩne na yi a Jopa pʋɔ ba a ba 'mataa chen.
44010024	Ba chen ka a wɛr tɩ chaar a ba ta a Sisariya, ka a ɩ a Konɩlɩyɔs mɩ chɛlɛ ba naa na wʋ bʋɔl a wʋ yir dẽme nɩ a wʋ barmɩne ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa a ba jɛ̃ gu.
44010025	Lɛ a Pita na ta kpɩɛrɛ a Konɩlɩyɔs yir wʋ ir tuor a Pita gbur dumo a wʋ niem na wʋ puor wʋ nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ.
44010026	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita nyɔɔ wʋ a wʋ ir, ka wʋ 'yɛr, "Ara, a maa mɩ nɩsaal lɛ n mɩ ɩ."
44010027	Wʋ 'yɛr wʋ naa lɛ tɩ kpɛ a die pɔ tɩ nyɛ nɩyɔɔ na duo.
44010028	A wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa an ba tara sɔr ɩka a sɩn Juu nɩbɛ ba lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a yɩn bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn wiil ma naa ɩka n taa bʋɔl nɩrɛ jaa nɩdɛɛr ɛ, bɩɩ nɩsɔ̃ɔ naa ɛ.
44010029	Ala lɛ so yɩn wa bʋɔl ma n ba baala ɛ, bɩɩ 'yɛr ɩka n kʋ̃ wa ɛ, bo 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ bʋɔl ma?"
44010030	Ka a Konɩlɩyɔs 'yɛr, "Ber anaar nɩ dɩna ɩn be a die pɔ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na bal baar. Ajienaa lɛ ka a ɩ daba na su fuu ka wʋ nyɩlɛ wa ara a n sɛ̃,
44010031	tɩ na wʋ bʋɔl ma, 'Konɩlɩyɔs, Nãaŋmɩn wõn a fʋ sʋɔrfʋ na wʋ tɩɛr a fʋ kʋfʋ fʋn kʋrɔ a nɔ̃n dẽme.
44010032	Tʋ̃ nɩrɛ a wʋ chen a Jopa tɩ bʋɔl Simon ban lɛ bʋɔlɔ Pita, wʋ be naa a daba ban bʋɔlɔ a Simon na nɔ̃nɔ̃ gãma ka a yir gbʋr man gogoro.'
44010033	Ala lɛ so ka n mɩ tʋ̃ a fɔɔ a lɛ nɛ bʋɔl fʋ, a fʋ mɩ pɛl pʋɔ tɩ wa. Pʋ̃pãanyã, Nãaŋmɩn niem lɛ sɩ jaa jɩ̃nɛ tɩ na chɛl bon jaa a sɩ Soro na tʋ̃n fʋ ɩka fʋ wa 'yɛr kʋ sɩ."
44010034	Ka a Pita pãa piel na wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Pʋ̃pãanyã n pãa bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn ba ooro ɛ.
44010035	Tɩchɛ wʋ ma den nɩbʋrɔ ba jaa na joro wʋ dãbɩ̃ɛ tɩ maal a lɛ na tor.
44010036	A 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩr kʋ a Isɩral nɩbɛ nɩ a nyã'maar 'yɛr na tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a bon jaa Soro sɛ̃.
44010037	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ala na ɩ a Judiya paal wʋ jaa na piel a Galilee a lɛ a Jɔɔn na wa mʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ 'yɛr baar.
44010038	Lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na ir a Yesu na yi Najaretɩ na wʋ de a wʋ Sɩɛ nɩ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ wʋ. Wʋ yɔn a ka wʋ jaa jilʋ̃ na wʋ maala vɩla sãana nɩ baalsɩ nɩ a bala jaa a dɛɛr sʋɔ na tara, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn ben a wʋ sɛ̃.
44010039	"Sɩn lɛ nyɛn nɩbir, a ala a jaa wʋn tʋ̃ a Juu nɩbɛ tẽn pɔ, nɩ a Jerusalɛm. Ba nyɔɔ wʋn kpa yɔɔl a daa ju ka wʋ kpi.
44010040	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn sɩ̃ɩ wʋ naa a kũu pɔ, a ber ata daar a wʋ ir ɩ vʋr na wʋ vɛ̃ a ba nyɛ wʋ.
44010041	Nɩbɛ ba jaa ba lɛ nyɛ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a sɩn na ɩ a dãasɩɛ dẽme a Nãaŋmɩn na de nie ir, sɩn nɩ 'lɔ 'mantaa di tɩ nyũ wʋn wa ir a kũu pɔ baar.
44010042	'Lɔ lɛ kpãkpãan sɩ ɩka sɩ mʋɔl 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ ɩka 'lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn ir ka wʋ ɩ a vʋɛ nɩ a kpĩisɩ 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ.
44010043	'Lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ba jaa 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr ɩka, nɩrɛ jaa wa sɔɔ de wʋ, wʋn nyɛn yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ tu a wʋ yuor pɔ."
44010044	Lɛ a Pita na chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ a anyãna, ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wa kpɛ a bala jaa na wõnõ a 'yɛr nyãna.
44010045	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bala na sɔɔ de na tu a Pita wa, nɛɛ 'maa ba naa a lɛ ban nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na pʋr a wʋ Sɩɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ.
44010046	A ba wõ ban 'yɛrɛ kɔkɔyor na ba pɛɛrɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn. Ka a Pita pãa 'yɛr,
44010047	"Nɩrɛ na tʋ̃ɔ ŋmaa a nɩbɛ banyãna sɔr ka ba ta so a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ɛ? Ba mɩ nyɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nɩtãa a sɩn."
44010048	Wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba naa ka ba so a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ nɩ Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor, a ba pãa sʋɔr a Pita ka wʋ be a ba sɛ̃ bɩ̃lãa.
44011001	A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a yɛɛr na be a Judiya wõ naa ɩka a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, mɩ sɔɔn a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr.
44011002	Lɛ a Pita na wa lɩɛb chen a Jerusalɛm a bala na ŋmaa a yʋɔr tɩ sɔɔl mii 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ 'yɛrɛ,
44011003	"Fʋ ben chen a bala na ba ŋmaa a yʋɔr yir tɩ lɔ̃ɔ din ba wɛ?"
44011004	Ka a Pita pãa piel mana a lɛ jaa na ɩ na wʋ kʋ ba,
44011005	"N ben a Jopa tẽe pɔ naa sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka a wa ɩ ma jaa de dee, ka n nyɛ nyɛfʋ kɔ̃ɔ. N nyɛn bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ fɩka fɔkpɛ̃ɛ ban tur bar ka wʋ yi saaju suu na wʋ gbũ jiir anaar ka wʋ suu wa ara a be ɩn be.
44011006	Be lɛ n muul kaa naa nyɛ dʋ̃gbɛɛ anaar jaa bʋrɔ na be ka a wɛr pɔ, mɔdʋ̃n, bʋ̃vʋʋrsɩ lɔ̃ɔn a lubil.
44011007	Ka n wõ kɔkɔr na 'yɛr, 'Pita ir na fʋ kʋ 'wɔb.'
44011008	Ka n haa 'yɛr, 'Kai, n Soro bon jaa na ɩ dɛɛr na ba vɩɛlɛ ɛ, ba kpɛ n nɛɛ pɔ jaa ɛ.'
44011009	Ka a kɔkɔr lɛ 'yɛr yi a saaju go, 'Ta bʋɔl bon jaa Nãaŋmɩn na maal a wʋ vɩɛlɛ bʋ̃dɛɛr ɛ.'
44011010	A anyãna ɩ naa nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ gbɛɛ ata tɩ lɛ tɔɔ a jaa don be a saaju go.
44011011	"Ajienaa, ka a ɩ a nɩbɛ ata ban tʋ̃ a n sɛ̃ na yi Sisariya mɩ tãn a yir 'lɔ pɔ ɩn kpɩɛrɛ dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ.
44011012	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr kʋ ma ka n tu ba chen naa taa baala ɛ. Maa nɩ a yɛɛr ayʋɔb banyãna lɛ 'mataa chen na sɩ tɩ kpɛ a daba yir.
44011013	A wʋ man kʋ sɩ a lɛ a malaka na wa a wʋ yir wa 'yɛr, 'Tʋ̃ nɩbɛ a Jopa ka ba tɩ bʋɔl daba na di Simon ban lɛ bʋɔlɔ Pita.
44011014	'Lɔ lɛ na waan 'yɛr wa 'yɛr kʋ fʋ ka a fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a fʋ yir dẽme ba jaa tu a 'yɛr 'lɔ pɔ nyɛ faafʋ.'
44011015	Ala lɛ ka n piel a 'yɛr naa 'yɛrɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wa a ba sɛ̃ a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ wa a sɩ sɛ̃ a pielfʋ.
44011016	Ka n pãa tɩɛrtɔ a lɛ a sɩ Soro na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, 'Jɔɔn den kʋ̃ɔ son, tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ Nãaŋmɩn na den a wʋ Sɩɛ son yɩ.'
44011017	Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ ba, a kʋfʋ bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ kʋ sɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto, maa mɩ nɩ ana, na ŋmaa Nãaŋmɩn sɔr?"
44011018	Ban wõ a anyãna, baa lɛ haa nɛɛ ɛ, tɩ pɛɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ, "Nãaŋmɩn pãa yuon sɔr kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka ban lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr nyɛ nyɛvʋr."
44011019	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ban kʋ a Sɩteven ka a pupuorbo bamɩne yɛ̃yɛl tɩ yi Fonisiya, Sipurusɩ nɩ Antiok, na ba mana a 'yɛr kʋrɔ a Juu nɩbɛ tɛɛ.
44011020	Ka a pupuorbo bamɩne na yi a Sipurusɩ nɩ a Sirenɩ, chen a Antiok na ba mɩ tɩ piel 'yɛrɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã kʋrɔ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ.
44011021	A sɩ Soro nũu dɔ̃ɔ pʋɔ ba ka a nɩyɔɔ dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ de na ba lɩɛb turo a sɩ Soro.
44011022	Ka a 'yɛr nyã lo a pupuorbo na be a Jerusalɛm toor pɔ, a ba ir Banabasɩ tʋ̃ a be Antiok.
44011023	Wʋn tɩ ta nyɛ a lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na wɩ̃ɛ ba, nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ wʋ naa ka wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ tɩ 'yɛr, ka ba ara nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a ba nyãa wʋ jaa kʋ a sɩ Soro.
44011024	Banabasɩ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ nɩsʋ̃ na sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na wʋ tara sɔɔfʋ na wʋ mɩ tɔɔ nɩyɔɔ waan a ba wa turo a sɩ Soro.
44011025	Ala puor lɛ ka a Banabasɩ pãa yɩ a be tu Tasusɩ tɩ bʋɔrɔ a Sɔɔl.
44011026	Wʋn tɩ nyɛ wʋ, ba lɩɛb wa Antiok na ba be be yuon gbul, ka a Banabasɩ naa Sɔɔl wile a nɩyɔɔ bala. Be a Antiok lɛ a pupuorbo nyɛ a yuor, "Kɩrɩsɩto turbo."
44011027	A sɔ̃ɔ nyãna lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ yi be a Jerusalɛm wa Antiok.
44011028	A ba ɩ̃sʋɔ yuor na di Agabus ir ara, ka Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɛ wʋ a wʋ 'yɛr, "Kɔ̃kpɛ̃ɛ na lon a Worom wɛr wʋ jaa." A kɔ̃ nyãna wa lo naa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Kɩlaudiyus na di a nãa.
44011029	A poturbo banyãna mɔ̃ naa na ba ir bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ lɛ a ba fɔ̃ɔ na jɩ̃ na ba sʋ̃ʋn a yɛɛr bala na be a Judiya.
44011030	Ban wa ir a kʋfʋ anyãna, Banabasɩ nɩ a Sɔɔl lɛ ba tʋ̃n a ba tɩ kʋ a nɩbɛrɛ.
44012001	A sɔ̃ɔ nyãna lɛ a Nãa Hɛrɔd nyɔɔr a pupuorbo bamɩne na wʋn ge.
44012002	Wʋ vɛ̃ naa ka ba ŋmaa Jemesɩ na ɩ a Jɔɔn yɛbɛ ju.
44012003	A Hɛrɔd nyɛn a lɛ ka a pɛl a Juu nɩbɛ pʋɔ, ka wʋ nyɔɔ a Pita mɩ. A anyãna ɩ naa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban tara a Paanʋ̃kõo Lɔ̃ɔfʋ.
44012004	Wʋn nyɔɔ a Pita a lɛ, a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ lɛ wʋ tɩ pɔɔ wʋ, tɩ na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ sojasɩ jiir anaar ka ba jʋrɔ taa kaara nɩ wʋ. Bojũu wʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka a Gõl Bar Difʋ wʋ po baar tɩchɛ ka wʋ tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr ka nɩrɛ jaa nyɛ.
44012005	Lɛ lɛ ba gu a Pita be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a pupuorbiir mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ wʋ.
44012006	A tɩ̃sɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a wɛr na chaar ka a Hɛrɔd na vɛ̃ ka ba waan a Pita ka wʋ tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr, bɔ̃jɔrsɩ ayi lɛ ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a Pita gbɛb sojasɩ ayi ka wʋ be a ba sãlsɔɔ gã guro, ka a sojasɩ bamɩne ara a pɔɔfʋ die dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ gu.
44012007	Ajienaa lɛ a sɩ Soro malaka wa kpɛ ara a wʋ sɛ̃ be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, ka a die wʋ jaa chaar. Ka a malaka ŋme a Pita jaa 'mɛ 'mɛ 'mɛ, sɩ̃ɩ wʋ 'yɛr, "Pɔɔ fɔɔ jaa ir," ka a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ for a Pita nũ'yɔ̃ɔ pɔ lo.
44012008	Be lɛ a malaka 'yɛr kʋ a Pita, "Su a fuu nɩ a nafɔbɔ na fʋ 'mɔɔ a fɔbaa vaar na fʋ turo nɩ ma." Ka a Pita ɩ a lɛ a malaka na 'yɛr.
44012009	Pita tu wʋn a lɛ tɩ yin a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, tɩchɛ nɩbir ba yuo wʋ a wʋ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a lɛ a malaka na 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ maala ɩn sɩrɛ ɛ, wʋ tɩɛr man tãa jãn lɛ wʋ jãna.
44012010	Ba tɩ yin a dɔ̃dɔr dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ pɔ, na ba lɛ tɩ yi a dɔ̃dɔr ayi sʋɔ pɔ, tɩ pãa ta a yõo dɔ̃dɔr a kur pãn na pɔɔ. Ban wa ta a wʋ yuo wʋ yõ a ba yi. A malaka tara na a Pita den a sɔr dẽdẽe ɩ̃sʋɔ chiin bɩ̃lãa tɩ bar wʋ tɩ chen ajienaa.
44012011	Ka Pita tɩɛr pãa yuo a wʋ 'yɛr, "Pʋ̃pãanyã n bɔ̃ɔn naa an ba ɩ baal ɛ, ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn lɛ tʋ̃ a wʋ malaka a wʋ wa 'loo ma faa a Hɛrɔd nũu pɔ, nɩ a lɛ jaa a Juu nɩbɛ na tɩɛr ɩka ba ge ma."
44012012	A anyãna wʋn wa tɩɛr yuo, wʋ chen a Mɛɛr na ɩ a Jɔɔn Maakɩ ma yir, be lɛ a pupuorbiir yɔɔ lɔ̃ɔ taa sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ wʋ.
44012013	Pita wa kpoor a yõo dɔ̃dɔr pãn, ka a gbãgbaa pɔɔbile ban bʋɔlɔ Woroda chen a pãn yuofʋ jie.
44012014	Wʋn wa wõ ka a ɩ Pita kɔkɔr lɛ ka a nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ wʋ tɩ põn bar, waa yuo a pãn ɛ, tɩ lɩɛb jo kpɛ a die pɔ tɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Pita lɛ be a yõo dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ!"
