44012015	A ba tãn wʋ pĩpĩi bar tɩ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Gelfʋ baal lɛ kpɛ fʋ!" Tɩ wʋ chɛnɛ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir 'yɛrɛ ɩka sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, ka ba 'yɛr, "A wʋ malaka tɔ̃ɔ lɛ."
44012016	Tɩchɛ ka a Pita chɛnɛ kpooro a pãn, ka ba tɩ yuo nyɛ ka a ɩ 'lɔ lɛ ka a nɛɛ 'maa ba.
44012017	Ka a Pita wɩlwɩl ba a nũu a ba bar gɔ̃n tɩchɛ ka wʋ man a lɛ a sɩ Soro na yin wʋ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ. Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba ɩka ba tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Jemesɩ nɩ a yɛɛr, na wʋ bar ba tɩ yi chen jiyuo.
44012018	A wɛr na chaar bibio, ka a sojasɩ ɩ chĩcham na ba sʋrɔ taa, "Bo lɛ na tara a Pita?"
44012019	Hɛrɔd vɛ̃n ka ba yɔbɔ wʋ faa na baa nyɛ wʋ ɛ, na wʋ kpãkpãan a sojasɩ mɩ faa tɩ 'yɛr ɩka ba kʋ ba. Ka a Hɛrɔd pãa yi a Judiya na wʋ chen a Sisariya na wʋ tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a be bɩ̃lãa.
44012020	A Hɛrɔd dɔ̃ɔ tara a Tire nɩbɛ nɩ a Sidon nɩbɛ nɩ jɛɛr, ka ba nyɛtaa nɛɛ na wa a nãa 'maalfʋ jie. Blastus na ɩ a nãa gbãgbaa wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sɛ̃ lɛ ba tʋ̃ ɩka wʋ 'maal a nãa kʋ ba bojũu a wʋ wɛr pɔ lɛ ba nyɛrɛ a ba bʋ̃diir.
44012021	Bɩbir kɔ̃ɔ, a Nãa Hɛrɔd sun a wʋ nafɔɔr jɩ̃nɛ nɩ a nãa dakɔɔ ju, na wʋn 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ.
44012022	Ka a nɩbɛ ŋmiere chɛlsɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Ŋmɩn kɔkɔr lɛ a nyãna na 'yɛrɛ, nɩrɛ ba lɛ ɛ."
44012023	Ajienaa lɛ ka a sɩ Soro malaka wa 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ baal bojũu waa de a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, ka a bufulo 'wɔb a nyaba ŋma ka wʋ kpi.
44012024	Tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr chɛnɛ yaara.
44012025	Lɛ a Banabasɩ nɩ a Sɔɔl na wa tʋ̃ a ba tʋ̃mɔ̃ baar a Jerusalɛm, ba tara naa Jɔɔn Maakɩ 'mataa chiin.
44013001	A Nãaŋmɩn puorbo bala na be a Antiok, ba tara naa bamɩne ka ba 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ka a bamɩne mɩ ɩ wiwiilbe, Banabasɩ nɩ Simeon ban bʋɔlɔ Nɩsɔɔlaa, Lusiyusɩ na yi a Sirenɩ tẽe pɔ, nɩ Manayen ban dɔ̃ɔ 'mataa guol a Nãa Hɛrɔd, nɩ a Sɔɔl.
44013002	A lɛ ban gal a kɔ̃ na ba sʋɔrɔ a sɩ Soro, ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ ir a Banabasɩ nɩ a Sɔɔl kʋ ma ka ba tʋ̃ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɩn bʋɔl ba."
44013003	A lɛ ban gal a kɔ̃ ba di bon jaa ɛ, ba dɔɔl ban a nuur sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ba tɩ bar ba sɔr ka ba chen.
44013004	A nɩbɛ ayi banyãna den a sɔr ka a Nãaŋmɩn de ba nie suun be a Selusiya na ba tɩ kpɛ a gboro chiine a Sipurusɩ.
44013005	Lɛ ban tɩ ta a Salamis, ba mʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr a be a Juu nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir. Ka a Jɔɔn Maakɩ be a ba sɛ̃ na wʋ sʋ̃nɔ̃ ba.
44013006	Ba yɔn a man dõdol wʋ jaa tɩ ta Pafos, be lɛ ba tuor a Juu nɩrɛ jɩbʋrɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ na ma ŋmara jirsɩ ka a wʋ yuor di Bar-Yesu.
44013007	Wʋ dɔ̃ɔ be a Segiyusɩ Pɔɔlusɩ na kaara a dõdol na ɩ yɛ̃ sʋɔ, a tẽkaara nyãna lɛ bʋɔl a Banabasɩ nɩ a Sɔɔl bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ wõ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr.
44013008	Tɩchɛ a Elimasɩ na ɩ a jɩbʋrɔ a wʋ yuor par lɛ a lɛ nɛ, ŋmaan a Banabasɩ nɩ a Sɔɔl sɔr ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka a tẽkaara nyãna wʋ sɔɔ a Yesu ɛ.
44013009	Ka a Sɔɔl nyãna ban bʋɔlɔ a Pɔɔl na sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kaara a Elimasɩ jaa tɩ̃ɩɩ tɩ wa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ.
44013010	"Fʋ ɩn Satan bie na fʋ ɩ bʋ̃sʋ̃n a jaa dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃. A fʋ pʋɔ sɛɛn naa bɛlfʋ nɩ bɛlfʋ 'yɛr bie, fʋ kʋ̃ bar a jir fʋn bʋɔrɔ ɩka fʋ sɔ̃ɔn a sɩ Soro sɔr dẽdẽe bar ɛ?
44013011	Pʋ̃pãanyã a sɩ Soro na ŋme fʋ naa ka fʋ jɔ̃ɔ tɩ tãn sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ, fʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ chãa ɛ." Ajienaa lɛ a Elimasɩ nɩbie de, ka a libe pɔɔ wʋ, ka wʋ bɔɔlɔ bʋɔrɔ nɩrɛ na nyɔɔ wʋ nũu.
44013012	A lɛ a tẽkaara na nyɛ a lɛ na ɩ, wʋ sɔɔn de, bojũu nɛɛ 'maa wʋ naa a lɛ ban wile a sɩ Soro yele.
44013013	Pɔɔl nɩ a wʋ taaba kpɛ̃n a gboro yi a Pafos chen be a Perga na be a Pamfiliya be lɛ a Jɔɔn Maakɩ tɩ bar ba tɩ lɩɛb chen a Jerusalɛm.
44013014	Ka ba yi a Perga chen Antiok na gbʋr a Pisidiya, a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir daar ba kpɛ̃n a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie na ba tɩ jɩ̃nɛ.
44013015	Ban wa kar a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ nɩ a ala a Nãaŋmɩn 'Yɛ'yɛrbɛ na sɛb baar, a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie nɩbɛrɛ sʋʋr naa Pɔɔl nɩ a wʋ taaba, "Yɛɛr, yɩn tara 'yɛr na sʋ̃ʋn a nɩbɛ sɩ kʋ yɩn sɔr, yɩ 'yɛr."
44013016	Ka a Pɔɔl vaa ir wɩlwɩl ba a nũu tɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Isɩral nɩbɛ woɩ, nɩ a yɩn na ba ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ɛ, na puoro a Nãaŋmɩn, yɩ chɛlɛ a lɛ ɩn 'yɛrɛ.
44013017	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã a sɩn Isɩral nɩbɛ na puoro lɛ dɔ̃ɔ chɛl ir a sɩ sãakpãmɩne na wʋ vɛ̃ ka ba dɔɔ paal be a Ijipitɩ pɔ. Kpɛ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ de faan ba yin a paal 'lɔ pɔ,
44013018	na wʋ bɔ̃ɔ tara ba be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ yuom lɩjaayi (40).
44013019	Paal bʋrsɩ ayopõi lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn dii bar be a Kanaan tɩ de a wɛr 'lɔ kʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ ka a ɩ ba sofʋ.
44013020	"A anyãna a jaa lɔ̃ɔn taa ɩ yuom kɔɔr anaar dɔɔl lɩjaayi nɩ pie (450). A anyã puor, Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ban 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ tɩ tãn a Samuwɛl na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ sɔ̃ɔ.
44013021	Be lɛ ka a nɩbɛ pãa wa sʋɔr Samuwɛl a wʋ bɔ nãa kʋ ba, ka Nãaŋmɩn de a Sɔɔl na ɩ a Kɩsɩ bidaba kʋ ba na ɩ a Benjamin bal nɩrɛ a wʋ ɩ a ba nãa yuom lɩjaayi (40).
44013022	Wʋn wa ir a Sɔɔl bar, wʋ den a David ka wʋ ɩ a ba nãa. Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa, 'N nyɛn a David na ɩ a Jesɩ bidaba ka a n ɩ̃gãn 'maa, wʋn maal yele a jaa ɩn bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ.'
44013023	"A Nãa David nyãna bal par pɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn ir a Fafaara Yesu kʋ a Isɩral nɩbɛ nɩtãa lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ.
44013024	Sɛrɛ tɩchɛ ka a Yesu wa, Jɔɔn mʋɔlɔ naa a tɩɛr lɩɛbfʋ 'yɛr na wʋ suoro a Isɩral nɩbɛ ba jaa a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
44013025	Lɛ a Jɔɔn na wa baaraa a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, 'An lɛ yɩ tɩɛr ɩka n ɩ naa? N ba ɩ a 'lɔ yɩn tɩɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ben a n puor waara, n ba sɛɛ ɩka n for a wʋ nafɔbɔ ɛ.'
44013026	"Maa yɛɛr na ɩ Abraham yɔn nɩ a yɩn na joro a Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ na ɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, sɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a faafʋ nyãna wa.
44013027	Bojũu, a nɩbɛ na be a Jerusalɛm nɩ a ba nɩbɛrɛ ba chɛl a Yesu ɛ, na ba 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ 'yɛr ka a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na sɛb a ba ma kara a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir jaa ɩ.
44013028	Ba gban ba dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ yele jaa na wiil ɩka wʋ sɛɛn kũu ɛ, tɩ ba sʋɔr a Pilate ɩka wʋ vɛ̃ ka ba kʋ a Yesu.
44013029	Ban wa maal a lɛ jaa ban sɛb a wʋ yele baar, a wʋ poturbo yɔɔ wʋn a daa ju na ba tɩ ũu a yaa pɔ.
44013030	Tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn ir wʋ a kũu pɔ.
44013031	A ber yɔɔ na wa po, a bala wʋn dɔ̃ɔ lɔ̃ɔ yɔn yin a Galilee tɩ tãn a Jerusalɛm, ba nyɛ wʋ naa, bala lɛ ɩ a dãasɩɛ dẽme a pʋ̃pãanyã kʋ a sɩ nɩbɛ.
44013032	"Sɩn 'yɛrɛ naa a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna kʋrɔ yɩ, a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne.
44013033	Nãaŋmɩn maal kʋ a sɩn na ɩ a yɔn a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne, na wʋ sɩ̃ɩ a Yesu yin a kũu pɔ. Nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Yiel Gãma ayi pɔ, 'Fʋ ɩ naa a maa bie, dɩna n lɩɛb a fʋ sãa.'
44013034	Lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a kũu pɔ nɩ nyã, wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ kpi pʋ̃ɔ go ɛ, a 'yɛr nyãna lɛ wʋ 'yɛr, 'Ɩn kʋ yɩ naa a yelsʋ̃n nɩ a sʋ̃ʋfʋ 'lɔ ɩn tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a David.'
44013035	A jie ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ 'yɛr ɩka, 'Fʋ kʋ̃ vɛ̃ ka a fʋ Chɛchɛ Sʋɔ kpɛ pʋ̃ɔfʋ jie ɛ.'
44013036	"A Nãa David na wa tʋ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ a wʋ sɔ̃ɔ, wʋ kpi naa ka ba ũu wʋ be a wʋ sãamɩne yar par, ka a wʋ ɩ̃gãn pʋ̃ɔ.
44013037	Tɩchɛ a 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na sɩ̃ɩ a kũu pɔ, ba kpɛ pʋ̃ɔfʋ jie ɛ.
44013038	"A lɛ jũu n yɛɛr, n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ka a tu naa a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ ka ba mʋɔl yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ kʋ yɩ.
44013039	A tu naa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɩka nɩrɛ jaa na sɔɔ de, Nãaŋmɩn na faa wʋn yin a ala a jaa a Mosesɩ Nɛɛ na kʋ̃ naa tʋ̃ɔ faa wʋ ɛ.
44013040	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, ka a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr taa wa a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ.
44013041	'Nyɛ a yɩn na kpɛrɛ, yɩ bʋ̃bʋr na yɩ wɛ, bojũu ɩn maal yele kɔ̃ɔ a yɩ sɔ̃ɔ yɩn ba be na sɔɔ de ɛ, ala ɩ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ gba 'yɛr kʋ yɩ.' "
44013042	Lɛ a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ na wa yire a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie, a nɩbɛ lɛ sʋɔr ba naa ɩka ba lɛ wa a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar wa 'yɛr a 'yɛr nyãna go.
44013043	Lɛ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ dẽme na wa yaar, a Juu nɩbɛ yɔɔ jie nɩ a bala na lɩɛb a Juu nɩbɛ turo naa Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ na ba bʋrɔ nɩ ba kpãkpãana ba 'yɛrɛ ka ba mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ nyã pɔ.
44013044	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir na lɛ wa ta, a tẽdẽme yɔɔ jie tɩ lɔ̃ɔn taa na wõ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr.
44013045	Lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ na nyɛ a nɩyɔɔ ba nyãna, nyuur kpɛ ba naa ka ba tʋrɔ chɩrɛ nɩ lɛ a Pɔɔl na 'yɛrɛ.
44013046	Ka a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ ba jo ba dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Sɩn 'lɔ, sɩn den nie 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ. Tɩchɛ yɩn ben tɔr bar na yaa kaa a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɩka yɩ sɛɛn naa a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ sɩn lɩɛb chen a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ sɛ̃.
44013047	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a sɩ Soro kpãkpãan sɩ ɩka sɩ ɩ, 'Ɩn maal fʋ naa ka fʋ ɩ chãa kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka fʋn chiin a faafʋ 'yɛr tɩ tãn a tẽe baaraa.' "
44013048	A lɛ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, na wõ a 'yɛr ba pʋɔ pɛl naa ka ba de 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr, ka a bala jaa a Nãaŋmɩn na ir ɩka ba nyɛ a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, sɔɔ de.
44013049	Ka a sɩ Soro 'yɛr yaar a paal 'lɔ wʋ jaa.
44013050	Tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ dam a pɔbɔ bala na turo a Juu nɩbɛ puorfʋ tɩ ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, nɩ a tẽe nɩdierbe 'yɔ̃ɔ ka ba dii a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ bar a paal 'lɔ pɔ.
44013051	Ka ba pɩ̃pɩ̃ a ba gbɛɛ tã-uul 'yɔ̃ɔ ba ka a wiil ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na ge ba naa tɩ na ba chen a Ikoniyum.
44013052	Ka a nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a poturbo bala ka ba sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ.
44014001	Be a Ikoniyum lɛ a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ ma chen a Juu nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie, be lɛ ba man a 'yɛr jaa nɛ nɛ nɛ ka a nɩyɔɔ bamɩne na ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, sɔɔ de a 'yɛr.
44014002	Tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bala na ba sɔɔ de ɛ, dam a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, sɔ̃ɔ a ba tɩɛr ka baa bara a yɛɛr ɛ.
44014003	Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ jɛ̃n a be na ba kor bɩ̃lãa, na ba 'yɛrɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr ba joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, ka a sɩ Soro mɩ̃ɛ wiil ɩka a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ na wʋ sʋ̃ʋ ba a ba tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ yelwiilsɩ nɩ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃.
44014004	Ka a tẽdẽme ŋma jiir ayi, a bamɩne pʋɔ a Juu nɩbɛ, ka a bamɩne mɩ pʋɔ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ.
44014005	Nɛchɩrɛ lon a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ nɩ a ba nɩbɛrɛ chara pɔ, ka ban maal Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ dɛɛr lɔb ba nɩ kʋsɩbɛ.
44014006	Tɩchɛ a ba bɔ̃ɔn na ba jo chen a tẽn anyãna na be a Likoniya paal pɔ, Lɩstɩra nɩ a Debi nɩ a tẽn ala na jilʋ̃ a be.
44014007	Be lɛ ba chɛnɛ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir na ba mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ.
44014008	A be a Lɩstɩra, dagbɛrɛ kɔ̃ɔ ben be ban lɔ̃ɔ dɔɔn ka waa chen kaa jaa ɛ.
44014009	Wʋ chɛlɛ naa lɛ a Pɔɔl na 'yɛrɛ ka a Pɔɔl kaa wʋ jaa tɩ̃ɩɩ nyɛ na wʋ bɔ̃ɔn wʋn tara sɔɔfʋ na sa.
44014010	A wʋ bʋɔl a daba 'yɛr, "Ir ara naa fʋ gbɛɛ." Ka a daba vaa ir na wʋ piel chiine.
44014011	Lɛ a nɩbɛ na wa nyɛ a lɛ a Pɔɔl na ɩ, ka ba ŋme chɛlma nɩ a Likoniya kɔkɔr pɔ, "A ŋmɩmɛ lɩɛb nɩbɛ suu wa a sɩ sɛ̃!"
44014012	Ba bʋɔlɔ naa a Banabasɩ "Jeyusɩ," na ba bʋɔlɔ a Pɔɔl mɩ "Hɛmɩsɩ," bojũu 'lɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a 'yɛ'yɛrɛ.
44014013	Ka a Jeyusɩ nyã puorfʋ yir na dɔ̃ɔ ara a tẽe kõkoor bɔɔrloro waan nɩ nadai nɩ a vapuulsɩ bojũu 'lɔ nɩ a nɩyɔɔ bala bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba lo bɔɔr kʋ ba.
44014014	Tɩchɛ lɛ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ, Banabasɩ nɩ a Pɔɔl na wa wõ a lɛ, ba tɔɔn a ba fuusɩ chɩɛr tɩ jo kpɛ be a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ tɩ tãna,
44014015	"Nɩbɛ, bãa lɛ yɩ maala a lɛ? Sɩn mɩ ɩn nɩbɛ, nɩsaalba a yɩ kaar. Sɩn waan naa a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã wa kʋ yɩ, na sɩ 'yɛrɛ yɩ ɩka, yɩ lɩɛb yi a yelpɔrsɩ anyãna pɔ, tɩ turo a Nãaŋmɩn vʋr. 'Lɔ lɛ maal a saaju, nɩ a tẽe, nɩ a man kpɛ̃ɛ, nɩ bon jaa na be be.
44014016	A kõr jaa wʋ dɔ̃ɔ bar ka nɩrɛ jaa turo a wʋ sɔr.
44014017	Tɩchɛ wʋ ma wiil a lɛ wʋn ɩ maal vɩla sʋɔ, na wʋ ma wiil a wʋ maal vɩla vɛ̃ ka a saa yi saaju waara, ka a bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ sɔ̃ɔ mɩ be be. Wʋ ma kʋ yɩn a bʋ̃diir yɔɔ ka yɩ pʋɔ pɛl."
44014018	A 'yɛr nyãna gba ban 'yɛr, tɩchɛ a chɛnɛ na ɩ tuo ka ban ŋmaa a nɩbɛ sɔr ka ban bar a bɔɔr lofʋ.
44014019	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bamɩne na pãa yi a Antiok nɩ a Ikoniyum wa tɔ̃n a nɩyɔɔ bala 'yɔ̃ɔ ka ba lɔb a Pɔɔl nɩ kʋsɩbɛ vu yin bar a tẽe kõkoor tɩɛr man tãa wʋ kpi naa.
44014020	Tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo tɩ ŋmaa jilʋ̃ wʋ ara nɩ ka wʋ ir kpɛ a tẽe pɔ. A wɛr na wa chaar ka 'lɔ naa Banabasɩ chen a Debi.
44014021	Be lɛ ba tɩ mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ, ka a nɩyɔɔ jaa sɔɔ turo a Yesu. A ba pãa lɩɛb chen a Lɩstɩra, Ikoniyum nɩ a Antiok,
44014022	tɩ mʋlɔ a pupuorbiir 'yɔ̃ɔn ba ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn ka ba ara nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ a sɔɔfʋ pɔ, na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Dɔɔyɛ yɔɔ pɔ lɛ sɩn tu tɩ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ."
44014023	Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ ir nɩdierbe kʋ ba a ba kaara a puorfʋ dẽme ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa. Ba gal kɔ̃ na ba sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn tɩ de ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro ban sɔɔ nũu pɔ.
44014024	Ba kpɛ̃n tala a Pisidiya, ba wa ta naa Pamfiliya,
44014025	ban wa mʋɔl a 'yɛr a Perga, ba suun chen be a Ataliya.
44014026	Be a Ataliya lɛ ba yi tɩ kpɛ a gboro chen a Antiok. Be lɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ de ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nũu pɔ ka wʋ sʋ̃ʋ ba, a ba tʋ̃ɔ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ a be tʋ̃ baar.
44014027	Ban tɩ tara jaa lɛ ba bʋɔl a pupuorbiir lɔ̃ɔ taa na ba man a lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn na de ba tʋ̃n nɩ a lɛ mɩ wʋn yuo sɔr kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka ba tʋ̃ɔ sɔɔ de.
44014028	Ba jɛ̃n a be kor bɩ̃lãa nɩ a poturbo.
44015001	Nɩbɛ bamɩne yin be a Judiya suun wa a Antiok wa wile a yɛɛr 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩn baa sɔɔ ka ba ŋmaa yɩ a yʋɔr nɩtãa lɛ a Mosesɩ na bin ɛ, yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ faafʋ ɛ."
44015002	A anyãna vɛ̃ naa ka a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ nɩ a nɩbɛ mĩi 'yɔ̃ɔ taa ka a ɩ nɛchɩrɛ. Be lɛ a ba ir Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ nɩ a pupuorbiir bamɩne 'yɔ̃ɔ ɩka ba chen a Jerusalɛm tɩ nyɛ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a 'yɛr nyãna.
44015003	A pupuorbiir na wa bar ba a sɔr, ba chen tɩ yi a Fonisiya nɩ a Samariya na ba man a lɛ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, na lɩɛb puoro a Nãaŋmɩn. Ka a yɛɛr ba jaa pʋɔ pɛl nɩ a 'yɛr nyã.
44015004	Ban wa ta Jerusalɛm, a pupuorbiir nɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ de ban nuur ayi, ka ba man a lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn na de ba tʋ̃n.
44015005	Ka a pupuorbiir bamɩne na chɛnɛ tara a Farasee wiilfʋ ir ara tɩ 'yɛr, "A nɩyor banyãna, a sɛɛ naa ka ban ŋma a ba yɔɩ na ba tu a lɛ a Mosesɩ na bin."
44015006	A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ lɔ̃ɔn taa na ban guor a 'yɛr nyãna.
44015007	A lɛ ban mana taa tɩ ta sɔ̃ɔ, Pita ir 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɛɛr, yɩ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ir man a yɩ pɔ, ka a bala na ba sɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, mɩ na wõ a faafʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr yi a n nɛɛ pɔ, na ba sɔɔ de.
44015008	Nãaŋmɩn na bɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ jaa nyãa lɛ wiil ɩka wʋ sɔɔn de ba na wʋ kʋ ba a wʋ Sɩɛ nɩtãa lɛ wʋn kʋ sɩ.
44015009	Waa maal a sɩn nɩ a bala ka sɩ tɛɛ taa ɛ, wʋ pɛɛn a ba nyãa ban sɔɔ jũu.
44015010	A lɛ jũu, bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ mʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ bɛɛr Nãaŋmɩn kaa, na yɩ tuo a poturbo tuor a sɩ sãakpãmɩne na ba dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃ɔ tuo ɛ?
44015011	Kai, sɩn sɔɔ naa ɩka a tu naa a sɩ Soro Yesu wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu lɛ sɩ nyɛ faafʋ nɩtãa a bala kaar."
44015012	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na duo ɩ jaa gbulo, tɩ chɛlɛ a lɛ a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ na mana a yelfɛrsɩ nɩ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn na de ba tʋ̃n a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bala pɔ.
44015013	Ban wa 'yɛr baar ka a Jemesɩ mɩ 'yɛr, "Yɛɛr, yɩ chɛlɛ ka.
44015014	Simon man kʋ sɩ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ tɩɛrtɔ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ ɩka wʋn ir nɩbɛ a ba pɔ, kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
44015015	Ka a lɛ na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ nɩ a 'yɛr nyã ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
44015016	'A anyã puor, ɩn lɩɛb tɩ mɛ a Nãa David yir 'lɔ na lo. Ɩn mɛn a 'lɔ na ŋmɛr, naa lɛ maal wʋ.
44015017	Ka a nɩbɛ bala na chɛ pãa na yɔ bɔ a Soro nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ na bʋɔlɔ a n yuor, lɛ lɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr na maal a yele anyãna,'
44015018	ka ba bɔ̃ɔn a kõr jaa jaa.
44015019	"Maa 'yɛr nɩ nyã ɩka sɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a ɩ tuo kʋ a nɩyor banyãna na lɩɛrɛ waara a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ.
44015020	Tɩchɛ yɩ ɩ a sɩ sɛb kʋ ba ɩka yaa, ba taa dire tɩɩ bon ɛ, na ba taa sɛ̃nɛ ɛ, dʋ̃ɔ na var kpi ba taa ɔɔrɔ ɛ, na ba taa ɔɔrɔ jɩ̃ɩ ɛ.
44015021	Bojũu, lɛ lɛ a Mosesɩ bin a nɛɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ ma mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr nyãna a tẽn a jaa ka ba mɩ ma kar naa a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar jaa."
44015022	Ka a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ lɔ̃ɔn a pupuorbiir ba jaa pãa kaa ir nɩbɛ a ba pɔ, ka ban 'matãan a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ tʋ̃ ka ba chen a Antiok. Judas ban bʋɔlɔ Basabasɩ nɩ Silasɩ lɛ ba ir, a nɩbɛ ayi banyãna mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ nɩbɛrɛ pʋɔ a yɛɛr.
44015023	Bala lɛ ba tʋ̃n a gãn nyãna, "A sɩn nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ na ɩ a yɩ yɛɛr puor naa a yɩn na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, na ɩ a sɩ yɛɛr be a Antiok nɩ a Siriya nɩ a Sɩlɩsɩya paal pɔ.
44015024	Sɩ wõn a bamɩne na yi a sɩ sɛ̃ sɩn ba kʋ ba sɔr ɛ, tɩ vuro yɩ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ yɩ 'yɛrɛ.
44015025	Ala lɛ so ka sɩ jaa sɔɔ ir nɩbɛ bamɩne tʋ̃ ka ban wa a yɩ sɛ̃, 'matãan a sɩ barmɩne Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ,
44015026	a nɩbɛ banyãna lɛ sɔɔ kũu a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor jũu.
44015027	A lɛ jũu lɛ sɩ tʋ̃n a Judas nɩ a Silasɩ ka ban tɩ man a ba nɛɛ a lɛ sɩn sɛb.
44015028	A vɩɛlɛ na kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nɩ a sɩn mɩ sɛ̃, ka sɩ kʋ̃ lɛ tuo yɩ tuor dɔɔl a anyãna ju ɛ.
44015029	Yɩ taa dire tɩɩ bon ɛ, yɩ taa ɔɔrɔ jɩ̃ɩ ɛ, na yɩ taa ɔɔrɔ dʋ̃ɔ na var kpi nʋ̃n ɛ, bɩɩ sɛ̃nɛ ɛ. Yɩ mɔ̃ na yɩ nyɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a yelsɩ anyãna pɔ. Yɩ jɛ̃ vɩla."
44015030	Ban wa bar a Pɔɔl, nɩ a Banabasɩ, nɩ a Judas nɩ a Silasɩ sɔr, ka ba suu chen be a Antiok, be lɛ ba tɩ lɔ̃ɔ taa a bala na puoro ba jaa na ba de a gãn kʋ ba.
44015031	A nɩbɛ na wa kar a gãn a 'yɔ̃ɔ ban ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn ka ba pʋɔ pɛl.
44015032	Judas nɩ a Silasɩ mɩ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ 'yɛr 'yɛr yɔɔ 'yɔ̃ɔn a yɛɛr ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
44015033	Ban wa jɛ̃ a be kor bɩ̃lãa, ka a yɛɛr lɛ bar ba sɔr nɩ nyã'maar ka ba lɩɛb chen a bala na tʋ̃ ba sɛ̃.
44015035	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl nɩ a Banabasɩ jɛ̃ be a Antiok, be lɛ a bala nɩ a ba taaba bamɩne wile tɩ mʋɔlɔ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr.
44015036	A mɩn lɛ wa kor bɩ̃lãa ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr kʋ a Banabasɩ, "Vɛ̃ ka sɩ lɛ chen tɩ piir a yɛɛr kaa a tẽn ala pɔ sɩn mʋɔl a sɩ Soro 'yɛr na sɩ kaa ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ba irɛ."
44015037	Ka a Banabasɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ de a Jɔɔn Maakɩ ka ba 'mataa chen.
44015038	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl ba tɩɛr ɩka a ba tara sɔr ɛ, bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ bar ba be a Pamfiliya ba lɛ pɔɔ ba chen a tʋ̃mɔ̃ jie ɛ.
44015039	Be lɛ ba tãn tãn taa na ba ŋma dẽdẽme, ka a Banabasɩ de a Jɔɔn Maakɩ na wʋ kpɛ̃n a gboro chiin be a Sipurusɩ.
44015040	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl mɩ ir a Silasɩ ka a yɛɛr de ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro nũu pɔ, ka wʋn sʋ̃ʋ ba.
44015041	Wʋ tun a Siriya nɩ a Sɩlɩsɩya 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bala na puoro ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
44016001	Pɔɔl tɩ chen a Debi na wʋ tɩ po chen a Lɩstɩra, be lɛ wʋ tɩ nyɛ a pupuoro ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Timoti ka a wʋ ma ɩ Juu nɩrɛ na wʋ puoro, tɩchɛ ka a wʋ sãa ba ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ ɛ.
44016002	Ka a yɛɛr na be a Lɩstɩra nɩ a Ikoniyum pʋr a Timoti yovɩla.
44016003	A Pɔɔl bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ tara wʋ 'mataa chiine na wʋ ŋmaa wʋ a yʋɔr, bojũu a Juu nɩbɛ na kpɩɛrɛ a be bɔ̃ɔn naa a Timoti sãa na ba ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ ɛ.
44016004	A lɛ ban lʋɔrɔ a tẽn, lɛ mɩ lɛ ba mana kʋrɔ ba lɛ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a nɩdierbe na be a Jerusalɛm na 'yɛr bin ka nɩbɛ ba turo.
44016005	Ba 'yɔ̃ɔn a pupuorbiir ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn ka a nɩbɛ mɩ waara pʋɔrɔ bɩbir jaa.
44016006	Pɔɔl nɩ a wʋ taaba tun a Fɩrgɩya nɩ a Galatiya paal pɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ŋmaa ba sɔr a ba taa mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr a be a Asɩya ɛ.
44016007	Ban wa gbʋr a Misiya wɛr pɔ, ba ta mʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba chen a Bitiniya tɩchɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ba kʋ ba sɔr ɛ.
44016008	A ba vɩɛ a Misiya bar tɩ suu chen be a Toroyas.
44016009	A tɩ̃sɔɔ lɛ a Pɔɔl nyɛ jãna pɔ, daba na yi Masedonɩya ara sʋɔrɔ wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Gɔ̃ɔ wa ka a Masedonɩya wa sʋ̃ʋ sɩ."
44016010	Pɔɔl na nyɛ a nyɛfʋ nyãna, sɩ ir chɔɔr a lɛ nɛ na sɩ chen a Masedonɩya, na sɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ bʋɔl sɩ a sɩ tɩ mʋɔl a wʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ ba.
44016011	A Toroyas sɩn yi tɔ̃ɔ kpɛ a gboro a dẽdẽe a lɛ nɛ chen a Samotɩrasɩ, ka a wɛr na wa chaar, sɩ tãn a Neapolis.
44016012	Be lɛ sɩ yin gbɛɛ chiin a Filipai, Worom dẽme lɛ dɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ a be na wʋ mɩ ɩ a Masedonɩya jikpɛ̃ɛ, be lɛ sɩ jɩ̃nɛ maal ber aŋmɩnɛ jaa.
44016013	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar, sɩ yin a tẽe pɔ suu a põn pɔ, be lɛ sɩ tɩɛr ɩka sɩn nyɛn jie ban ma sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn. Sɩ jɩ̃nɛ naa be na sɩ piel 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr kʋrɔ pɔbɔ na lɔ̃ɔ a be.
44016014	A pɔbɔ banyãna na chɛlɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ yuor din Lidiya na yara fɔjɩɩr, na wʋ yi a Tayatira tẽe pɔ, wʋ mɩ puoro naa Nãaŋmɩn. A sɩ Soro yuon a wʋ tɩɛr ka wʋ sɔɔ de a lɛ a Pɔɔl na 'yɛr.
44016015	'Lɔ nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa na wa so a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, wʋ bʋɔl sɩ naa a sɩ wa a wʋ yir a wʋ wa 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ yɩ sɔɔ naa ɩka n sɔɔn de a sɩ Soro, sɩrɛ jaa yɩ wa jɛ̃ a n yir." Lɛ lɛ wʋ mʋlɔ sɩ.
44016016	Daar kɔ̃ɔ sɩn lɛ chiine a jie 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jie, sɩ tuor gbãgbapɔɔbile na tara a sɩdɛɛr na wʋ ma 'yɛrɛ yele na ɩ daar kɔ̃ɔ. A lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ na wʋ nyɛrɛ libiyɔɔ kʋrɔ a bala na so wʋ.
44016017	Ka a pɔɔbile nyãna turo a Pɔɔl na wʋ turo sɩ tãna 'yɛrɛ, "A nɩbɛ banyãna ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na be saaju tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ na ba wile yɩ a faafʋ sɔr."
44016018	Lɛ lɛ a pɔɔbile mar bɩbir jaa ka a Pɔɔl wa vʋʋr faa tɩ lɩɛb 'yɛr kʋ a sɩɛ 'lɔ na be a pɔɔbile pɔ ɩka, "Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor pɔ, n 'yɛr kʋ fʋ ɩka fʋ wa yi a pɔɔbile pɔ." Ajienaa ka a sɩɛ yi tɩchɛ wʋ bar.
44016019	A pɔɔbile sorbo na wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka baa lɛ nyɛrɛ tɔ̃nɔ̃ a pɔɔbile sɛ̃ ɛ, ba nyɔɔn a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ tɔɔ chiin be a daa pɔ a nɩbɛrɛ niem.
44016020	Ba chiin ban tɩ kʋ a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ tɩ 'yɛr, "A nɩbɛ banyãna ɩ naa a Juu nɩbɛ na ba wa kpɛ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sɩ a tẽe.
44016021	Ba tara na yelsɩ kɔ̃ɔ an ba tara sɔr kʋ a sɩn Worom nɩbɛ a sɩn sɔɔ bɩɩ maal ɛ."
44016022	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala ir pʋɔ na baa bara a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ ɛ, ka a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ vɛ̃ ka ba yaar a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ fuusɩ bar tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba fɔb ba.
44016023	A lɛ ban wa fɔb ba sɛɛ, ba nyɔɔr ban 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a 'lɔ na guro a pɔɔfʋ die, a wʋ bɔ̃ɔ kaara ba.
44016024	Wʋn wõ a nɩtɔ̃, wʋ tɩɛ ban 'yɔ̃ɔ a die 'lɔ na be a sãlsɔɔ tɩ lũ a ba gbɛɛ mar daa.
44016025	A tɩ̃sɔɔ bɩ̃ɩn lɛ a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn, na ba yiele nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn yiel, ka a ba taaba ban lɔ̃ɔ pɔɔn ba chɛlɛ.
44016026	Ajienaa ka a tẽe dam kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, ka a pɔɔfʋ yir par kparaa mɩ dam. Ka a pɔɔfʋ der dɔ̃dɔɩ yuo yuor a jaa, ka nɩrɛ jaa bɔ̃jɔrma ban lũn wʋ for for.
44016027	Ka a 'lɔ na guro a pɔɔfʋ die jɛɔ ir na wʋ nyɛ a lɛ a pɔɔfʋ der dɔ̃dɔɩ na yuor, ka wʋ vʋ̃ɔ sɔɔ ɩka wʋ kʋ̃n wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, bojũu wʋ man tãa a pɔɔfʋ dẽme yin jo.
44016028	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl tãn, "Ta ge fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, sɩ jaa ben ka."
44016029	A wʋ bʋɔl a ba waan fɩ̃tɩn wa kʋ wʋ a wʋ pɔɔ kpɛ̃n be a die pɔ, na wʋ tɩ lo gbur dumo mɩrɛ a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ niem.
44016030	Tɩ pãa ir tara ba yin tɩ sʋʋr, "Nɩbɛrɛ, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ɩn ɩrɛ wa nyɛ faafʋ?"
44016031	A ba 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro Yesu, fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a fʋ yir dẽme na nyɛn faafʋ."
44016032	Be lɛ ba pãa 'yɛr a sɩ Soro 'yɛr kʋ wʋ nɩ a bala jaa na be a wʋ yir.
44016033	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a pɔɔfʋ die guguro de ba yin a tɩ̃sɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na wʋ tɩ pɛɛ a ba natɩɛ tɩchɛ a ba mɩ tɔ̃ɔ so a 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
44016034	Ka a pɔɔfʋ die guguro tara ba kpɛ̃n a wʋ yir tɩ maal bʋ̃diir kʋ ba, ka nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a wʋ yir dẽme, bojũu 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa sɔɔn de a Nãaŋmɩn.
44016035	Wɛr na wa chaar a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ ir a ba tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ tʋ̃ na ba 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chen tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a 'lɔ na guro a pɔɔfʋ die ɩka, a wʋ yuo a dɔɔr bala bar."
44016036	Ka a pɔɔfʋ die guguro 'yɛr kʋ a Pɔɔl, "A 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ tʋ̃n ɩka n yuo a fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a Silasɩ bar. A lɛ pʋ̃pãanyã yɩn tʋ̃ɔ chiine, yɩ chiine nɩ nyã'maar."
44016037	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr kʋ a bala ban tʋ̃, "Chãa pɔ jaa lɛ ba vɛ̃ a ba fɔb sɩ, baa tɔɔr a sɩ 'yɛr ɛ, sɩ gba ɩ naa a Worom dẽme tɩ ba 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ. Pʋ̃pãanyã a ba lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba sɔɔl yuo sɩ bar? Bala mɩ̃ɛ ba wa yuo sɩ bar."
44016038	A tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ na tɩ man a lɛ kʋ a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ, ban wa wõ ɩka a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ ɩ naa Worom dẽme, dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba naa.
44016039	Ka a bala mɩ̃ɛ pãa chen tɩ 'maal ba yin a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, tɩ sʋɔr ba ɩka ba yi a tẽe 'lɔ pɔ.
44016040	Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ na wa yi a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, ba chen a Lidiya yir, be lɛ ba tɩ tuor a yɛɛr ka ba 'yɔ̃ɔ ba ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn tɩ pãa yi a be chen.
44017001	Ba tun a Amfipolis nɩ Apoloniya na ba wa a Tɛsalonika, be lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir be.
44017002	Lɛ a Pɔɔl na ma irɛ lɛ wʋ chen be a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir, Pɛ̃nfʋsɩ gbɛɛ ata jaa lɛ wʋ kpɛ a be ka a 'lɔ nɩ a bala vɩɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãma.
44017003	Wʋ mana na wile a lɛ an sɛɛ a Nɩ-iraa na di dɔɔyɛ tɩ na wʋ ir a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋr, "A Yesu nyãna ɩn ben 'yɛrɛ a wʋ 'yɛr, lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa."
44017004	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bamɩne sɔɔ a lɛ na ba pʋɔ a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ, 'matãan a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ puoro a Nãaŋmɩn lɔ̃ɔn pɔɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnsɩ.
44017005	Tɩchɛ ka a nyuur kpɛ a Juu nɩbɛ, ka ba bɔ a ba taaba nɩbomo be a daa pɔ lɔ̃ɔ taa, na ba piel gɔ̃mɔ̃ be a tẽe pɔ. Ba tɩ sɛɛn a Jason yir bʋɔrɔ a Pɔɔl nɩ a Silasɩ ɩka ba yin chiin ba a nɩyɔɔ bala niem.
44017006	Tɩchɛ ban ba wa tɩ nyɛ ba ɛ, ba nyɔɔn a Jason nɩ a yɛɛr bamɩne chiin a tẽe nɩbɛrɛ niem tɩ tãna 'yɛrɛ. "A dɔɔr banyãna lɛ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wɛr wʋ jaa, ba wa tãn ka pʋ̃pãanyã
44017007	ka a Jason tuor de ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ yir. Ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ naa a Nãa Siisa chire na ba 'yɛrɛ ɩka nãa ɩ̃sʋɔ ben be ban bʋɔlɔ Yesu."
44017008	A lɛ a tẽe nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a nɩyɔɔ bala na wõ a 'yɛr nyãna, a dam ba naa.
44017009	A ba pãa 'yɔ̃ɔ a Jason nɩ a yɛɛr bala a ba yab libie tɩ ba bar ba sɔr.
44017010	A lɛ a wɛr na wa tɔ̃ɔ sɔb, ka a yɛɛr bar a Pɔɔl nɩ Silasɩ sɔr ka ba chen be a Beriya. Ban tɩ ta, ba chen be a Juu nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir.
44017011	A Juu nɩbɛ bala na be a Beriya ɩn chɛchɛlbɛ gar a bala na be a Tɛsalonika, bojũu ba den a 'yɛr nɩ chɩlfʋ na ba vɩɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãma kaara bɩbir jaa ɩka ba kaa lɛ a Pɔɔl na 'yɛrɛ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ bɩɩ.
44017012	A Juu nɩbɛ yɔɔ jie sɔɔn de a 'yɛr lɔ̃ɔn a bala na ba ɩ Juu nɩbɛ dɔɔr yɔɔ jie, nɩ a pɔɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnsɩ bamɩne yɔɔ jie.
44017013	A Juu nɩbɛ na be a Tɛsalonika na wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Pɔɔl ben a Beriya mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr, ba chen a be tɩ chãgbala a nɩbɛ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ ba.
44017014	Ka a yɛɛr mɩ tɔ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Pɔɔl a man sɔr a wʋ chen, tɩchɛ ka a Silasɩ nɩ a Timoti 'lɔ jɛ̃ be a Beriya.
44017015	A nɩbɛ bala na bɩɛl a Pɔɔl ba tɩ tãn wʋn a Atensɩ, bala lɛ wʋ lɩɛb tʋ̃ ɩka a Silasɩ nɩ a Timoti a ba wa fɔɔ a wʋ sɛ̃.
44017016	A lɛ wʋn chɛnɛ chɛlɛ ba be a Atensɩ, suur wa tɩ kpɛ wʋ naa a lɛ wʋn nyɛ a tẽe na sɛɛn a tɩbɛ.
44017017	Lɛ lɛ 'lɔ nɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a Greek bala na puoro a Nãaŋmɩn ma mana taa be a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir, nɩ a bala wʋn ma pɔɔ a daa pɔ bɩbir jaa nɩ nɩrɛ jaa wʋn tuor.
44017018	Ka a bɔ̃bɔ̃ɔnbɔ bamɩne na yi a Epikuriya nɩ a Sɩtoyik gbul pɔ piel chɩrɛ nɩ a Pɔɔl. Ka a bamɩne sʋrɔ, "Bo lɛ a dabʋlɔbʋlɔ nyãna ara 'yɛrɛ?" Ka a bamɩne mɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Ŋmɩn sãansɩ kɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr lɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ." Ba 'yɛrɛ naa nɩtɔ̃ bojũu, Pɔɔl mʋɔlɔ naa a Yesu 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nɩ a kũu pɔ irfʋ 'yɛr.
44017019	Be lɛ ba pãa bʋɔl wʋ chiin be a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie a Areyopagusɩ na ba 'yɛr, "Fʋn tʋ̃ɔ wiil sɩ a fʋ wiil paalaa nyãna fʋn wile a sɩ bɔ̃ɔ bɩɩ?
44017020	'Yɛr sãan lɛ a nyã fʋn waan a sɩ wõnõ na sɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ bɔ̃ɔ a par."
44017021	Atensɩ dẽme ba jaa lɔ̃ɔn a sãanba na kpɩɛrɛ a be, baa tara tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ pʋɔ a 'yɛr paalaa ban ma 'yɛrɛ na ba chɛlɛ nɩ yelpaalaa na ɩrɛ.
44017022	Lɛ lɛ a Pɔɔl pãa ir a nɩbɛ na lɔ̃ɔ a Areyopagusɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Atensɩ dɔɔr, n nyɛn bɔ̃ɔn yɩn nʋ̃ ŋmɩmɛ puorfʋ.
44017023	Bojũu ɩn yʋɔrɔ kaara a yɩ tɩbɛ jiir, n tɩ nyɛn a bɔɔr lofʋ jie ɩ̃sʋɔ yɩn sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ, ŊMƖN 'LƆ SƖN BA BƆ̃Ɔ Ɛ. A Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ gba yɩn mɩ̃ɛ na puoro tɩ ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ n waan ɩka n wa mʋɔl kʋ yɩ.
44017024	"A Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ na maal a wɛr nɩ a bomo a jaa na be a pɔ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a saaju nɩ a tẽe jaa Soro, na waa gãna a yie ala a nɩbɛ na mɛn a ba nuur kʋ wʋ ɛ.
44017025	Waa dɩɛl nɩrɛ nũu tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala ɩ wʋ bʋɔrɔ na bon kɔ̃ɔ ɛ, bojũu 'lɔ mɩ̃ɛ lɛ kʋ nɩrɛ nyɛvʋr, ka wʋ vʋrɔ nɩ bon jaa.
44017026	Dabʋ̃'yen pɔ lɛ wʋ tu na wʋ maal a nɩbʋrsɩ, ka ba kpɩɛrɛ a wɛr wʋ jaa. A wʋ man a sɔ̃ɔsɩ kʋ ba, nɩ a jiir ala ban na kpɩɛrɛ.
44017027	Nãaŋmɩn maal naa nɩtɔ̃ ka nɩrɛ na tʋ̃ɔ yɔbɔ wʋ, amɩne sɛ̃ ban nyɛ wʋ naa, bojũu waa jãan a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ɛ.
44017028	'Bojũu, a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ sɩ chɛnɛ na sɩ be ka a tẽe pɔ,' na sɩ yʋɔrɔ nɩtãa lɛ a yɩn mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ bamɩne na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, 'A wʋ bibiir lɛ sɩ ɩ.'
44017029	"Sɩn ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir jũu, yɩ taa ɩ a sɩ tɩɛr ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn nyã kaara naa fɩka bon nɩrɛ na de wʋ yɛ̃ bɩɩ bɔ̃ɔfʋ mɛn, sɛlma, bɩɩ libipɩla, bɩɩ kʋsɩr kaar ɛ.
44017030	A kõr jaa 'lɔ, Nãaŋmɩn lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ ba bɔ̃ɔfʋ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ, wʋ kpãkpãana na nɩrɛ jaa jie jaa ɩka, ba lɩɛb ba tɩɛr.
44017031	Bojũu wʋ ir bɩbir bin wʋn na de a daba 'lɔ wʋn ir, na wʋ tɔɔr a wɛr 'yɛr nɩ yeltorsɩ pɔ. Wʋ vɛ̃n ka a chaar kʋ nɩrɛ jaa wʋn sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a kũu pɔ."
44017032	Ban wa wõ a kũu pɔ irfʋ 'yɛr, bamɩne lan wuol, tɩchɛ ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩn bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka sɩ lɛ wõ a 'yɛr nyã nɩdaar."
44017033	A lɛ, Pɔɔl bar ba naa a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie.
44017034	Tɩchɛ ka a nɩbɛ bɩ̃lãa turo a Pɔɔl na ba sɔɔ de a 'yɛr, a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ Diyonɩsɩs na ɩ a Areyopagusɩ lɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩrɛ, ka a pɔɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ na pʋɔ yuor di Damarisɩ nɩ bamɩne mɩ na pʋɔ.
44018001	A anyã puor, Pɔɔl yin a Atensɩ na wʋ chen be a Korɩntɩ.
44018002	Be lɛ wʋ tuor a Juu nɩrɛ na di Akuila na wʋ ɩ Pontus bal nɩrɛ, 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ pɔɔ Pɩrɩsɩla na yi a Itali wa a ba kor ɛ, bojũu a Nãa Kɩlaudiyus 'yɛr naa ɩka a Juu nɩrɛ jaa wʋ yi a Worom. Ka a Pɔɔl chen ɩka wʋ piir ba kaa.
44018003	Wʋ tɩ jɛ̃n a be a ba 'mataa tʋ̃nɔ̃ bojũu ba jaa bɔ̃ɔn a gãma tʋ̃mɔ̃.
44018004	A Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar jaa Pɔɔl ma chen a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir ma tɩ 'yɛrɛ a 'yɛr bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ lɩɛb a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ tɩɛr.
44018005	Lɛ a Silasɩ nɩ a Timoti na wʋ yi a Masedonɩya wa a Korɩntɩ, Pɔɔl den a wʋ sɔ̃ɔ wʋ jaa na wʋ mʋɔlɔ mana kʋrɔ a Juu nɩbɛ ɩka a Yesu lɛ a Nɩ-iraa.
44018006	Tɩchɛ ka Juu nɩbɛ 'yɛrɛ a Pɔɔl kpõkpoor 'yɛr, a wʋ pɩ̃pɩ̃ a fɔbaa 'yɔ̃ɔ ba tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A yɩ jɩ̃ɩ a lɩɛb dɔɔl a yɩ ju, a ba lɛ ɩ maa 'yɛr ɛ, an yi dɩna chiine, n chiine naa a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ jie."
44018007	Pɔɔl yin be a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir na wʋ gʋɔr a daba ɩ̃sʋɔ na di Titiyusɩ Jusɩtusɩ na ba ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ ɛ na puoro ka a wʋ yir gbʋr a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir.
44018008	Ka a Kɩrɩsɩpusɩ na ɩ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir nɩdiere nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro 'yɛr nɩ a Korɩntɩ dẽme yɔɔ na wõ a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr, a ba sɔɔ a wʋ so ba jaa a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ.
44018009	A tɩ̃sɔɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ, a sɩ Soro 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ a Pɔɔl jãna pɔ ɩka, "Taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr ta pɔɔ nɛɛ ɛ.
44018010	Bojũu, ɩn pʋɔ fʋ naa, nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ nyɔɔ fʋ bɩɩ maal fʋ dɛɛr ɛ, bojũu n chɛnɛ na tara nɩyɔɔ a tẽe nyã pɔ."
44018011	Be lɛ a Pɔɔl jɛ̃ a be a Korɩntɩ yuon gbul nɩ bʋ̃ŋmaa na wʋ wile ba a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr.
44018012	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a Galio ɩ a Akaya nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, ka a Juu nɩbɛ guor taa na ba nyɔɔ a Pɔɔl chiin be a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie.
44018013	Be lɛ ba tɩ 'yɛr, "A daba nyãna lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ lɩɛb a nɩbɛ tɩɛr ka ba puoro Nãaŋmɩn na ba tu a lɛ a sɩ nɛbinsɩ na 'yɛr ɛ."
44018014	Ka a Pɔɔl haa nɛɛ ɩka wʋ 'yɛr 'yɛr, tɩchɛ ka a Galio 'yɛr kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ, "A yɩn, ala ta ɩ yeldɛɛr bɩɩ yelbier kɔ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ, ɩn taa 'maan ɩ̃gãn chɛlɛ.
44018015	Tɩchɛ an ben wa lɔ̃ɔ taa nɩ a yɩ 'yɛr bie nɩ yoe 'matãan a yɩ nɛbinãa yɩn mɩ̃ɛ yɩ maal, maa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ a 'yɛr nyãna tɔɔr ɛ."
44018016	Lɛ lɛ wʋ vɛ̃ a ba dii ba bar be a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie.
44018017	A ba lɩɛb nyɔɔ a Sosetenesɩ na ɩ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na ba ŋme be a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ yir dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ, tɩchɛ a Galio baka ba be be ɛ.
44018018	Pɔɔl jɛ̃n be a Korɩntɩ tẽe kor bɩ̃lãa, tɩ pãa bar a yɛɛr na wʋ kpɛ a gboro chiine a Siriya ka a Pɩrɩsɩla nɩ a Akuila pɔɔ wʋ. Sɛrɛ tɩchɛ ka wʋ chen, wʋ vɛ̃n ka ba põ wʋ a ju be a Senkereya, bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ põl 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
44018019	Ba tãn be a Efesus tẽe pɔ, ka a Pɔɔl bar a Pɩrɩsɩla nɩ a Akuila tɩ na wʋ mɩ̃ɛ chen be a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie ka a 'lɔ naa Juu nɩbɛ tɩ mana taa.
44018020	A ba sʋɔr wʋ ka wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a be bɩ̃lãa tɩ waa sɔɔ ɛ.
44018021	Tɩchɛ wʋn wa chiine wʋ tɩr nɛɛ kʋ ba, "Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn wa sɔɔ naa, ɩn lɩɛb wa." Be lɛ wʋ kpɛ a gboro yi a be a Efesus tẽe pɔ.
44018022	Wʋn tɩ ta a Sisariya wʋ don be a Jerusalɛm na wʋ tɩ puor a bala na puoro, tɩ pãa suu chen a Antiok.
44018023	Pɔɔl na tɩ jɛ̃ a be a Antiok kor bɩ̃lãa, wʋ pãa yin yʋɔrɔ a Galatiya paal 'lɔ wʋ jaa nɩ a Fɩrgɩya na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a poturbo ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
44018024	Ka a Juu nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ yuor na di Apolosɩ yin be a Aleksandiriya na wʋ wa a Efesus tẽe pɔ. Wʋ ɩ naa nɩrɛ na jãn na wʋ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn gãma tɩ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr sʋ̃.
44018025	Apolosɩ nyã dɔ̃ɔ jãn a sɩ Soro sɔr defʋ, na wʋ 'yɛrɛ nɩ nɩbijɩɛ na wʋ wile nɩ Yesu yele ka a tor, tɩchɛ ka a ɩ Jɔɔn Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ tɛɛ lɛ wʋ bɔ̃ɔ.
44018026	Wʋ piel na wʋ 'yɛrɛ nɩ nyãa be a Juu nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔfʋ yir. A Pɩrɩsɩla nɩ a Akuila na wa wõ a wʋ 'yɛr, ba bʋɔl wʋn be a ba yir na ba pãa wiil wʋ a Nãaŋmɩn sɔr jaa dẽ dẽ.
44018027	Apolosɩ wa bʋɔrɔ naa Akaya chenfʋ, ka a yɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ tɩ sɛb gãn kʋ a bala na puoro a be a ba de wʋ. Wʋn tɩ ta a be a ɩn sʋ̃ʋfʋ kpɛ̃ɛ kʋ a bala a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ na vɛ̃ ka ba sɔɔ de a Yesu.
44018028	Wʋ 'yɛr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa lɔb a Juu nɩbɛ chãa pɔ, na wʋ chɩrɛ ba yuoro nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn gãma wile ba ɩka a Yesu lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa.
44019001	Lɛ a Apolosɩ na chɛnɛ be a Korɩntɩ, Pɔɔl den a mɔgɔ̃ɔ sɔr na wʋ tɩ ta a Efesus tẽe pɔ. Be lɛ wʋ nyɛ a poturbo bamɩne,
44019002	na wʋ sʋʋr ba, "A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ yɩn sɔɔ de a Yesu, yɩ nyɛn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ bɩɩ?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Kai, saa gba wõ ɩka Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ben be ɛ."
44019003	Ka a Pɔɔl sʋʋr ba, "Tɩ kɔ̃buor lɛ yɩ so?" Ka ba 'yɛr, "Jɔɔn kʋ̃ɔ lɛ sɩ so."
44019004	A Pɔɔl 'yɛr kʋ ba, "A bala na lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr lɛ a Jɔɔn so ba Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ ɩka ba sɔɔ de a 'lɔ na waara a wʋ puor, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Yesu."
44019005	A nɩbɛ na wa wõ a anyãna ba sɔɔ naa ka wʋ so ba a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor.
44019006	Ka a Pɔɔl dɔɔl ba a wʋ nuur ka Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wa kpɛ ba a ba 'yɛrɛ kɔkɔyor, na ba ma piel 'yɛrɛ lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na wiil ba.
44019007	Ban ɩn dɔɔr pie nɩ ayi.
44019008	Ŋmɛrsɩ ata lɛ wʋ be a be na wʋ ma kpɩɛrɛ a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie na wʋ ma kpɩrkpɩrɛ ba wile ba a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr.
44019009	Tɩchɛ a bamɩne kpɛ̃mɛ naa a ba nyãa na ba tɔr baa sɔɔ ɛ, tɩ na ba kpɛrɛ a Sɔr. Ka a Pɔɔl bar ba, tɩ na wʋ ma tara a bala na sɔɔ de, ma kpɛ̃n be a Tiranusɩ jãnfʋ diyal 'lɔ pɔ, a ba ma tɩ mana taa.
44019010	Lɛ lɛ wʋ tara tɩ tãn yuom ayi, ka a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ, bala jaa na be a Asɩya paal pɔ wõn a sɩ Soro 'yɛr.
44019011	Nãaŋmɩn den a Pɔɔl tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃yɔɔ.
44019012	A Pɔɔl fɔbile wʋn ma fɩɛlɛ nɩ nyĩe nɩ a wʋ pẽpele ala wa sɩɩr baalaa, a baalsɩ ba jaa ma sa naa, ka a sɩdɛbɛ ma yire a nɩbɛ pɔ.
44019013	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ bamɩne mɩ yi yʋɔrɔ na dii a sɩdɛbɛ ka a yi na ba fere de a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a bala na tara a sɩdɛbɛ, "A Yesu 'lɔ a Pɔɔl na mʋɔlɔ, a wʋ yuor pɔ lɛ sɩ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ wa yi."
44019014	A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na di Sekeva dabil ayopõi lɛ dɔ̃ɔ maala a lɛ nɛ.
44019015	Daar kɔ̃ɔ a sɩdɛɛr sʋʋr ba naa, "N bɔ̃ɔn Yesu naa bɔ̃ɔ Pɔɔl, tɩchɛ a yɩn mɩ ba boo yɩ ɩ?"
44019016	Ka a daba 'lɔ na tara a sɩ dɛɛr pãa ɔɔ nyɔɔr ba jaa, na wʋ ŋme ba jaa pɩrpɩr tɔɔr a ba bonsɩ chɩɛr ka ba jo yi a die pɔ nɩ sal'mɔi.
44019017	A Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ, na kpɩɛrɛ a be Efesus tẽe pɔ, ba jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa a yele nyãna, ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba a baa lɛ tara a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor dɩ̃ɛnɛ nɩ ɛ.
44019018	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na sɔɔ de, yi chãa pɔ, na ba 'yɛrɛ a ba maal dɛbɛ.
44019019	A jɩbʋʋrbɔ bala mɩ na sɔɔ, waan naa a ba jɩbʋʋrgãma wa chʋm a nɩbɛ ba jaa niem, ban wa sɔr a gãma ala ban chʋm libie ka a ɩ libipɩla turo ayi dɔɔl lɩjaayi nɩ pie (50,000).
44019020	A sɔr nyãna lɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr yaar de jie wʋ jaa nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ.
44019021	A anyãna a jaa na wa ɩ, Pɔɔl ŋmen nyãa ɩka wʋn chen a Jerusalɛm na wʋn tu a Masedonɩya nɩ Akaya, "Maa wa ta a be baar, ɩn chen a Worom mɩ."
44019022	Wʋ tʋ̃ naa a nɩbɛ ayi a bala na sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ Timoti nɩ Erastus ka ba chen a Masedonɩya, tɩchɛ ka a 'lɔ jɩ̃nɛ be a Asɩya paal pɔ kor bɩ̃lãa.
44019023	A sɔ̃ɔ nyãna lɛ a damfʋ ir a Sɔr tʋfʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
44019024	Sãa kuro kɔ̃ɔ yuor na di Demetirus, wʋ ma den a kpãna na wʋ kur a Atemisɩ puorfʋ yirbil ka a bala na ɩ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ nyɛrɛ libie.
44019025	A Demetirus bʋɔl a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa nɩ a bala jaa mɩ na bɔ̃ɔ a maalfʋ na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɛɛr, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa tɔ̃nɔ̃ sɩn nyɛrɛ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ nyã pɔ.
44019026	Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ nyɛ naa na yɩ wõ a lɛ a Pɔɔl nyãna na 'yɛrɛ na wʋ lɩɛrɛ a nɩyɔɔ tɩɛrsɩ a ka Efesus tẽe pɔ, nɩ a Asɩya wɛr wʋ jaa. Wʋ 'yɛr naa ɩka a ŋmɩmɛ ala ban maal nuur ba ɩ ŋmɩmɛ ɛ.
44019027	A ba ɩ a sɩ yara na lo tɛɛ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ ba kʋ̃ lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Atemisɩ puorfʋ yir kpɛ̃ɛ go ɛ. Ka a Asɩya nɩ a wɛr wʋ jaa kʋ̃ lɛ puoro a ŋmɩn pɔɔ nyã go ɛ."
44019028	Ban wõ lɛ a Demetirus na 'yɛr, ka a suur nyɔɔ ba a ba tãna 'yɛrɛ, "A sɩn Efesus ŋmɩn Atemisɩ bɛrma naa."
44019029	Ajienaa lɛ a tẽe wʋ jaa pɔɔn gɔ̃mɔ̃, ka a nɩbɛ nyɔɔ a Gayus nɩ Aristakus, Pɔɔl tʋ̃tʋ̃taaba lɛ a ba 'mataa yi a Masedonɩya na ba ŋmʋr ba a lɛ chiin a jie 'lɔ a tẽe nɩbɛ na ma lɔ̃ɔ dɩ̃ɛnɛ.
44019030	Ka a Pɔɔl mɩ ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ daa yi a be a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a poturbo ba sɔɔ ɛ.
44019031	A nɩbɛrɛ bamɩne gba na yi a paal 'lɔ pɔ na ɩ a Pɔɔl barmɩne, tʋ̃n nɩbɛ ka ba sʋɔr wʋ ɩka wʋ taa ɩrɛ wa yire be a dɩ̃ɛn jie ɛ.
44019032	Burbur kpɛ̃n a nɩyɔɔ bala na duo a be, ka bamɩne 'yɛrɛ turo nɩ ka sɛn, ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛrɛ turo nɩ jɩ̃ yuo, ka bamɩne mɩ gba ba bɔ̃ɔ bo 'yɔ̃ɔ ban be be ɛ.
44019033	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ daa Aleksanda 'yɔ̃ɔ be a niem, ka a nɩyɔɔ bala tãna mana wʋ lɛ wʋn na 'yɛr. Wʋ wɩlwɩl ban nuur ɩka, ba bar gɔ̃n tɩ wʋ 'yɛr a ba kaa.
44019034	Tɩchɛ ban wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Juu nɩrɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ, ba jaa ŋmen chɛl bʋ̃'yen lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ na ba 'yɛrɛ, "A sɩn Efesus ŋmɩn Atemisɩ bɛrma naa."
44019035	A tẽe gãn sɛɛrɛ vɛ̃n ka a nɩyɔɔ bala ŋmaa vʋʋr tɩ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Efesus dẽme woɩ, a wɛr wʋ jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a Efesus tẽe lɛ kaara a Atemisɩ kpɛ̃ɛ nyã puorfʋ yir a wʋ kʋsɩr 'lɔ na yi a saaju lo.
44019036	A nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ jũu, nɩrɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ chɩɩr ɛ, yɩ ɩ jaa gbul na yɩ ta pɔɔrɔ yelsɩ ɛ.
44019037	A nɩbɛ banyãna yɩn waan a kana ba ju bon jaa a puorfʋ yir ɛ, bɩɩ 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛɛr jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ ŋmɩn pɔɔ nyã ɛ.
44019038	Ala ɩ a Demetirus nɩ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ wa tara nɩrɛ nɩ 'yɛr, a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ bɩbie ben be nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ ban tʋ̃ɔ chen a be tɩ bʋɔl taa.
44019039	Ala ɩ yele kɔ̃ɔ mɩ ben be a yɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ 'yɛr, ban tʋ̃ɔ maal a be a nɩyɔɔ ba jaa niem.
44019040	A lɛ an sɩ ben 'yɛr pɔ, a damfʋ nyã na dam a dɩna jũu. A 'yɛr nyãna jũu, saa be jaa na tʋ̃ɔ wiil a par ɛ, bojũu a ba tara par ɛ."
44019041	A anyãna wʋn 'yɛr baar tɩ na wʋ wɛl a nɩyɔɔ bala bar.
44020001	Lɛ a gɔ̃mɔ̃ na wa baar, Pɔɔl tʋ̃n bʋɔl a poturbo ka ba wa, a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn tɩ bar ba tɩ chen a Masedonɩya.
44020002	Be lɛ wʋ tu a tẽn ala pɔ na wʋ 'yɛr 'yɛr yɔɔ 'yɔ̃ɔn a bala na puoro ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn na wʋ tɩ tãn a Greek wɛr pɔ,
44020003	wʋ jɛ̃n a be ŋmɛrsɩ ata. Bojũu a Juu nɩbɛ dɔ̃ɔ guoro taa a wʋ yele, ala lɛ so waa lɛ kpɛ a gboro chen a Siriya ɛ, tɩ na wʋ lɩɛb tu a Masedonɩya sɔr nɩ gbɛɛ.
44020004	Ka a bala na pʋɔ wʋ a ba 'mataa chen lɛ, Sopater a wʋ sãa lɛ Pirihusɩ na yi Beriya, Aristakus nɩ Sekundusɩ mɩ na yi Tɛsalonika, Gayus na yi Debi nɩ Timoti nɩ Tɩchɩkusɩ nɩ a Torofimusɩ na yi a Asɩya paal pɔ.
44020005	A nɩbɛ banyãna lɛ de nie tɩ chɛlɛ sɩ be a Toroyas.
44020006	Tɩchɛ a Paanʋ̃kõo Lɔ̃ɔfʋ di na wa baar, sɩ kpɛ̃n a gboro yi be a Filipai tẽe pɔ na sɩ maal ber anũu tɩ na sɩ pɔɔ ba a be Toroyas jɩ̃nɛ a be ber ayopõi.
44020007	A Pɛ̃nfʋ divɩɛ bio daar jãanʋɔr, sɩ jaa lɔ̃ɔn taa na sɩn 'mataa di. Pɔɔl 'yɛrɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋrɔ a nɩbɛ bojũu wɛr wa chaar, wʋn chen naa. Wʋ 'yɛr kor jaa ka wɛr tɩ põ.
44020008	A be a bɔɔpɩɛ pɔ sɩn lɔ̃ɔ ba chʋm fɩ̃tɩnsɩ yɔɔ bin.
44020009	Pɔlbile kɔ̃ɔ yuor na di Yutikus jɩ̃nɛ naa a tokoro nɛɛ ka a gʋ̃ɔ kpɛ wʋ. Lɛ a Pɔɔl na 'yɛr kor a wʋ gur jaa chɩ̃ɩɩ na wʋ yi a be a saaju faa lo a be tẽe, bojũu ba mɛn a bɔɔpɩɛ dɔɔl taa ata ka ba suu 'mɔɔ ka ɩ wʋ kpi naa.
44020010	A Pɔɔl suun tɩ lo bib a kũu tɩ kõr wʋ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ, "Yɩ ta kõnõ ɛ, wʋ chɛnɛ na vʋrɔ."
44020011	Wʋ pãa don be a bɔɔpɩɛ pɔ, ka wʋ tɩ ŋma a paanʋ̃ɔ ka ba 'mataa di tɩ wʋ lɛ 'yɛr lɛ̃ɛɛ ka wɛr tɩ chaar ka wʋ yi a be chen.
44020012	Tɩchɛ ka pɔlbile ir kpɛ̃mɛ ka ba ɩ̃gãn 'maa a ba tara wʋ kul a yir.
44020013	Sɩn den nie kpɛ a gboro na sɩ chiine a Asosɩ, be lɛ sɩn tɩ 'mɔɔ a Pɔɔl, lɛ lɛ wʋ dɔ̃ɔ man sɩ tɩ chiine nɩ gbɛɛ a be.
44020014	Lɛ wʋn tɩ tuor sɩ a be Asosɩ, sɩ 'mɔɔ wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ a gboro pɔ na sɩ chiine be a Mitilene.
44020015	Wɛr na wa chaar, sɩ yin a be tɩ ta Kiyosɩ ka a wɛr lɛ bɔ̃ɔ chaar sɩ go kaa ɩ sɩ vɩɛn Samosɩ bar. A ber ata daar lɛ sɩ pãa ta a Miletusɩ.
44020016	Pɔɔl bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ po a Efesus tẽe bar na wʋ ta gã be a Asɩya paal pɔ ɛ, bojũu wʋ bʋɔrɔ na fɔɔ ɩka 'lɔ tʋ̃ɔ, wʋ ta a Jerusalɛm a Pentikosɩ bɩbir daar.
44020017	Pɔɔl na chɛnɛ be a Miletusɩ lɛ wʋ tʋ̃ bʋɔl a bala na puoro a be a Efesus, a ba nɩdierbe ka ba wa.
44020018	Ban wa ta, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ bɔ̃ɔ lɛ ɩn be dɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ a yɩ sɛ̃, yi a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ jaa ɩn wa a Asɩya paal pɔ.
44020019	Mɩ̃ɛ siirfʋ nɩ nɩbikʋ̃ɔ lɛ n tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a sɩ Soro tʋ̃mɔ̃, bojũu a Juu nɩbɛ ba maal ma vɩla ɛ.
44020020	Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka n ba sɔɔl yɩ yele jaa na sʋ̃ʋ yɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ n wile yɩn chãa pɔ, nɩ a yɩ yie pɔ.
44020021	N kpãkpãan naa a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ɩka ba lɩɛb wa a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, na ba lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro Yesu.
44020022	"Pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ, Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr man ka n chiine a Jerusalɛm, n ba bɔ̃ɔ lɛn na tɩ pɔɔ ma a be ɛ.
44020023	Yelbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ n bɔ̃ɔ ɩka, tẽe jaa pɔ, a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ma vɛ̃n ka n bɔ̃ɔn ɩka die pɔ pɔɔfʋ, nɩ wõm lɛ ɩn tɩ tuor.
44020024	Tɩchɛ a anyãna maa bã ma ɛ, ala ɩ ɩn tʋ̃ɔ jo ta a baaraa naa tʋ̃ a lɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu na kʋ ma a tʋ̃mɔ̃, ɩka n 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ.
44020025	"Yɩ nyɛ, pʋ̃pãanyã a yɩn bala jie ɩn yɔ naa mʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr, yɩ kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ ma go ɛ.
44020026	A lɛ jũu, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ a dɩna ɩka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa bɔr, n nũu ba pʋɔ be ɛ.
44020027	Bojũu n ba dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔl yɩ yele jaa ɛ, tɩ man a lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ kʋ yɩ.
44020028	Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a nɩbɛ bala 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na maal yɩ a yɩ ɩ a nɩdierbe. Yɩ kaara a Nãaŋmɩn pupuorbiir bala wʋn dãn a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ jɩ̃ɩ.
44020029	N bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka maa wa chen baar, nɩbɛ na lɩɛb gbõgboi kpɛ a yɩ pɔ, ba kʋ̃ bar yɩ ɛ.
44020030	Bamɩne na yin a yɩn mɩ̃ɛ pɔ gba, na ba jɛr a yelmɩ̃ɛ bɛl nɩbɛ ka ba turo ba.
44020031	A lɛ jũu yɩ guro yɩ mɩ̃ɛ na yɩ tɩɛr kaa, yuom ata nɩ nyã ɩn ba vɛ̃ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wiilfʋ ɛ, nɩbikʋ̃ɔ lɛ n wile nɩ yɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ.
44020032	"Pʋ̃pãanyã, n de yɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nũu pɔ, nɩ a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ 'yɛr bie pɔ, a yɩ na tʋ̃ɔ nʋ̃ɔ a wʋ kʋ yɩ a bʋ̃sʋ̃n ala wʋn tara kʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ.
44020033	N ba tara nyuur nɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa libir, bɩɩ sɛlma, bɩɩ a fɔɔr ɛ.
44020034	Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a n bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ, a n nũu pɔ lɛ a yi, naa sʋ̃ʋ a bala ɩn lɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ.
44020035	Bon jaa ɩn maal, n wiil yɩ naa ɩka a tʋ̃kpɩ̃ɛn a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ lɛ, sɩn tu na sɩ sʋ̃ʋ a nɩbaalsɩ, yɩ tɩɛrɛ a lɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, 'An ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n kʋ a 'lɔ na de bon kʋ nɩrɛ, gar a 'lɔ na de.' "
44020036	Wʋn 'yɛr a anyãna baar, wʋ gbur dumo ka ba jaa 'mataa sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn.
44020037	Ba jaa ŋman nɩbikʋ̃ɔ tɩ na ba kõr kõr wʋ.
44020038	A lɛ na maal sɔ̃ɔ a ba pʋɔ nɩ nyã, a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr ɩka ba kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ wʋ go ɛ, tɩ na ba bɩɛl wʋ suun a gboro jie.
44021001	Sɩn wa bar taa baar, sɩ kpɛ̃n a gboro na sɩ tor a Kos a dẽdẽe a lɛ nɛ, a wɛr na wa chaar ka a ɩ sɩ tãn a Worodesɩ yi a be chen a Patara.
44021002	Sɩ nyɛn a gboro ɩ̃sʋɔ na chiine a Fonisiya ka sɩ kpɛ chiine.
44021003	Sɩn wa nyɛrɛ a Sipurusɩ tẽe sɩ lan wʋn bar a guba jie tɩ ta a Siriya tẽe pɔ. Tire lɛ sɩ ta ara an ɩ be lɛ a gboro na wɛl a tuor wʋn tuo.
44021004	Be lɛ sɩ nyɛ a poturbo bamɩne na sɩ jɩ̃nɛ a ba sɛ̃ ber ayopõi. Ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ tu a ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba 'yɛr kʋ a Pɔɔl ɩka wʋ taa chiine a Jerusalɛm ɛ.
44021005	Tɩchɛ a sɩ bɩbie na wa ta, sɩ yin de a sɩ sɔr. Ka a poturbo bala ba jaa nɩ a ba pɔbɔ nɩ a ba bibiir ba jaa bɩɛl sɩ yin a tẽe pɔ, tɩ tãn a man gogoro nɛɛ, ka sɩ gbur dumo sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn.
44021006	Sɩn wa bar taa baar, sɩ kpɛ̃n a gboro pɔ, tɩ ba mɩ lɩɛb kulo a yir.
44021007	A Tire sɩn be yi, a man pɔ lɛ sɩ chen bɩ̃lãa tɩ ta a Tolemaisɩ be lɛ sɩ puor a yɛɛr bamɩne na be be na sɩ gã a be bɩbir bʋ̃'yen.
44021008	Sɩn ir a be chiine sɩ tãn be a Sisariya na sɩ chen a Filip na mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ na wʋ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ ayopõi bala ɩ̃sʋɔ ban dɔ̃ɔ ir be a Jerusalɛm yir.
44021009	Wʋ dɔ̃ɔ tara pɔɔsarsɩ anaar na ba kul sɩrbɛ ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn ma kʋ ba a wʋ 'yɛr a ba 'yɛrɛ.
44021010	Sɩ jɛ̃n a be kor bɩ̃lãa ka a Agabus yi be a Judiya na,
44021011	wʋn wa a sɩ sɛ̃. Wʋ den a Pɔɔl sɩɛ gãn na wʋ lũn a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nuur nɩ a gbɛɛ tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr. "A Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr naa, 'Nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ na be a Jerusalɛm na lũ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na so a sɩɛ gãn nyãna, na ba 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nuur pɔ.' "
44021012	A lɛ sɩn wõ a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ ka a sɩn nɩ a nɩbɛ bala na be a be 'mataa sʋɔr a Pɔɔl ɩka wʋ taa chiine a Jerusalɛm ɛ.
44021013	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "Bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩ kõnõ na yɩ chɩrɛ ma a ɩ̃gãn a lɛ? N sɔɔ naa, a ta ɩ a lũfu tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ n kpi be a Jerusalɛm a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor jũu."
44021014	A lɛ sɩn sʋɔr wʋ faa sɩ mɩ bar naa tɩ 'yɛr "A sɩ Soro bɔfʋ a ɩ."
44021015	A anyã puor lɛ sɩ chɔɔr na sɩ do be a Jerusalɛm.
44021016	Ka a poturbo bala na be a Sisariya bɩɛl sɩ na ba waan sɩ a daba 'lɔ na di a Minason yir be lɛ sɩn wa kpɩɛrɛ, Sipurusɩ tẽe pɔ lɛ wʋ yi tɩ na wʋ ɩ a poturo kor.
44021017	A lɛ sɩn wa ta a Jerusalɛm, a yɛɛr de sɩn nuur ayi.
44021018	Ka a wɛr na wa chaar, sɩn nɩ a Pɔɔl jaa 'mantaa chen ɩka sɩ tɩ nyɛ a Jemesɩ ka a ɩ be lɛ a nɩbɛrɛ ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa.
44021019	Pɔɔl na puor ba jaa baar, wʋ man naa yele a jaa kʋ ba, a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na de wʋ tʋ̃n be a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ pɔ.
44021020	A lɛ ban wõ anyãna ba jaa pɛɛn Nãaŋmɩn tɩ na ba pãa 'yɛr kʋ a Pɔɔl, "Yɛbɛ faa nyɛ, a Juu nɩbɛ turo turo na sɔɔ de, tɩchɛ ba chɛnɛ na tara nɩbijɩɛ nɩ a nɛbinãa.
44021021	Ba man kʋ ba ɩka fʋ̃ʋ lɛ wile a Juu nɩbɛ bala na kpɩɛrɛ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ pɔ, ka ba taa turo a Mosesɩ ɛ, na fʋ lɛ wile ɩka ba taa ŋmara a ba bibiir yɔɩ ɛ, na ba taa ɩrɛ a lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ na ma ɩrɛ ɛ.
44021022	Ban wõn ɩka fʋ wan a ka, ŋmɩnɛ sɩn ɩ?
44021023	Fʋ̃ʋ bʋɔrɔ fʋ tu a lɛ sɩn na 'yɛr. Dɔɔr anaar ben ka a sɩ sɛ̃ na ba põl 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ.
44021024	De a nɩbɛ banyãna na fʋ pʋɔ ba, a yɩ tɩ pɔl a fʋ yab a ba jur põfʋ sãma. Ka nɩrɛ jaa na pãa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a lɛ ban man 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ ba ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ mɩ turo naa a nɛbinãa.
44021025	Tɩchɛ a nɩyor bala na sɔɔ de, sɩ sɛb gãn kʋ ba a lɛ sɩn 'yɛr ɩka, ba taa dire tɩbɛ bomo ɛ, bɩɩ ɔɔrɔ jɩ̃ɩ ɛ, bɩɩ 'wɔb dʋɔ na var kpi ɛ, na ba taa sɛ̃nɛ ɛ."
44021026	Wɛr na wa chaar, Pɔɔl den a dɔɔr anaar bala ka ba 'mataa tɩ pɔl a ba mɩ̃ɛ. Tɩ na wʋ pãa chen be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir na tɩ 'yɛr a bɩbie ala a ba pɔlfʋ na baar nɩ a bɔɔrlo bomo ala a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na ir.
44021027	A lɛ a ber ayopõi na wa gbʋrɔ a baarfʋ, a Juu nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi a Asɩya paal pɔ nyɛn a Pɔɔl a be Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir, na ba dam a nɩyɔɔ bala a ba nyɔɔ wʋ.
44021028	Ba gboolo naa, "Isɩral nɩbɛ woɩ, yɩ wa sʋ̃ʋ sɩ yooo. A daba lɛ anyãna na wile a nɩbɛ jie jaa ka ba kpɛrɛ a sɩ nɩbɛ nɩ a nɛbinãa lɔ̃ɔn a jie nyãna. Lɛ tɛɛ gba ba lɛ ɛ, wʋ tara na a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, kpɛ̃n ka a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir na wʋ sɔ̃ɔ a jivɩla nyãna."
44021029	Ba dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ a Torofimusɩ na yi a Efesus nɩ a Pɔɔl a ba tɩɛr man tãa a Pɔɔl tara wʋn kpɛ̃n be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir.
44021030	A tẽdaa wʋ jaa kab, ka a nɩbɛ yire a tẽe wʋ jaa joro waara na ba wa nyɔɔ a Pɔɔl. Ba nyɔɔ wʋn a lɛ tɔɔ yin a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir jie tɩ pɔɔ a pãma ajienaa.
44021031	Ka ba ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba kʋ a Pɔɔl ka a yele tɩ ta a Worom sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɩka a Jerusalɛm wʋ jaa dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ naa.
44021032	A wʋ vaa ir a lɛ na wʋ tara a nɩbɛrɛ bamɩne nɩ a sojasɩ na wʋ suu chiin be a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ. Lɛ ban wa nyɛ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a wʋ sojasɩ a ba bar a Pɔɔl ŋmefʋ.
44021033	Lɛ a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na wa ta wʋ tɩ nyɔɔn a Pɔɔl na wʋ vɛ̃ ka ba gbãr wʋ nɩ bɔ̃jɔrsɩ ayi. Tɩ pãa sʋʋr ɩka nɩ ana lɛ, nɩ bo lɛ wʋ maal.
44021034	Bamɩne na be a nɩyɔɔ bala pɔ 'yɛrɛ na turo nɩ jiyuo ka bamɩne mɩ 'yɛrɛ turo nɩ jiyuo a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na ba nyɛ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, a gɔ̃mɔ̃ jũu, wʋ vɛ̃n ka ba tara a Pɔɔl gʋɔr be a sojasɩ kpɛfʋ jie.
44021035	Lɛ a Pɔɔl na wa ta a dofʋ jie a nɩbɛ pir pirfʋ jaa waa naa ka a sojasɩ 'mɔɔ a Pɔɔl.
44021036	Ka a nɩyɔɔ bala na turo tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩ kʋ wʋ."
44021037	Lɛ a sojasɩ na wa ɩka ba kpɛ̃n a Pɔɔl a be a ba kpɛfʋ jie wʋ sʋɔr naa a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɩka, "N 'yɛr 'yɛr kɔ̃ɔ kʋ fʋ bɩɩ?" Ka a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sʋʋr wʋ, "Fʋn tʋ̃ɔn 'yɛr a Greek kɔkɔr bɩɩ?
44021038	A ba ɩ fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a Ijipitɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ ŋmaa a jɛɛr na fʋ tɔɔ dɔɔr turo anaar (4,000) kpɛ̃n be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ ɛ?"
44021039	Ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "N ɩ naa Juu nɩrɛ naa yi a Tasusɩ na be a Sɩlɩsɩya paal pɔ, naa yi a tẽe nyãna pɔ nɩrɛ jaa na bɔ̃ɔn, yãayãabɩlɛ sɔɔ ka n 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ."
44021040	A sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kʋn a Pɔɔl sɔr, ka a wʋ ir ara a dofʋ jie, na wʋ wɩlwɩl a nɩyɔɔ bala a nuur ka ba bar gɔ̃mɔ̃. A lɛ ban wa ŋmaa a vʋʋr wʋ den a ba Juu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr na 'yɛrɛ nɩ.
44022001	"N yɛɛr nɩ n sãamɩne yɩ chɛlɛ a n 'yɛr ɩn 'yɛrɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã."
44022002	A lɛ ban wa wõ wʋn 'yɛrɛ nɩ a ba mɩ̃ɛ Juu nɩbɛ kɔkɔr ka ba jaa ŋma vʋrɔ, tɩ a Pɔɔl pãa 'yɛrɛ,
44022003	"Maa ɩn Juu nɩrɛ ka ba dɔɔ ma a Tasusɩ na be a Sɩlɩsɩya paal pɔ, tɩchɛ a kana a Jerusalɛm lɛ ba guol ma. A wiwile Gamaliel pĩlem lɛ n jɩ̃nɛ ka wʋ wiil ma a nɛɛr ala a sɩ sãakpãmɩne na dɔ̃ɔ turo ka n mɩ turo a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a n nyãa wʋ jaa, nɩtãa a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na be turo a dɩna.
44022004	N gen a nɩbɛ bala na turo a Sɔr nyãna naa kʋ, n nyɔɔr dɔɔr nɩ pɔbɔ jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ.
44022005	A bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ na tʋ̃ɔn di ma dãasɩɛ, ba sɛ̃ lɛ n de gãma na chiin a ba yɛɛr sɛ̃ be a Damaskus, n chen ɩka n tɩ nyɔɔr a nɩbɛ banyãna waan a Jerusalɛm ka ba kpãa ba.
44022006	"Mɔ̃tɔ̃tuo sɔ̃ɔ lɛ n chiine tɩ gbʋrɔ a Damaskus, ajienaa ka ɩ chãa yin be a saaju na wʋ wa chaar jilʋ̃ ma.
44022007	Ka a n tɔ̃ɔ lo a tẽe a lɛ nɛ tɩ naa wõ kɔkɔr na sʋrɔ ma, 'Sɔɔl, Sɔɔl, bo lɛ fʋ gere ma a lɛ?'
44022008	Ka n sʋʋr, 'Soro, an lɛ fʋ ɩ?' Ka a kɔkɔr 'yɛr, 'Maa lɛ a Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ a 'lɔ fʋn gere.'
44022009	A maa nɩ a bala na lɔ̃ɔ chiine ba nyɛn a chãa, tɩchɛ baa bɔ̃ɔ a nɩnyɩnɛ kɔkɔr lɛ wʋn 'yɛrɛ nɩ ma par ɛ.
44022010	Ka n sʋʋr, 'Soro, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ɩn ɩ?' Ka a Soro 'yɛr, 'Ir na fʋ kpɛ be a Damaskus tẽe pɔ, be lɛ ban tɩ man fʋ a lɛ ɩn bʋɔrɔ ɩka fʋ ɩ.'
44022011	Ka n lɔ̃ɔturbo bala nyɔɔ ma a nũu tɔɔ kpɛ̃n be a Damaskus tẽe pɔ, bojũu a chãa 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na chaar 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a lɛ nɛ n ba lɛ nyɛrɛ ɛ.
44022012	"Daba kɔ̃ɔ yuor na di Ananias wan ɩka wʋ wa nyɛ ma, wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn puoro na wʋ turo a nɛbinãa ka a Juu nɩbɛ ba jaa na kpɩɛrɛ a be 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ.
44022013	Wʋ wa ara na gbɛb ma tɩ 'yɛr, 'N yɛbɛ Sɔɔl, lɛ nyɛrɛ,' ka a ɩ ajienaa ka a ɩ n nyɛ wʋ naa.
44022014	Be lɛ wʋ pãa 'yɛr kʋ ma, 'A sɩ sãakpãmɩne Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ir fʋ ɩka fʋ bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ, na fʋ lɛ nyɛ a chɛchɛ sʋɔ 'lɔ, na fʋ wõ a 'yɛr bie yi a wʋ nɛɛ pɔ.
44022015	Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ na ɩ a dãasɩɛ sʋɔ na fʋ kʋ a nɩbɛ ba jaa, a ala fʋn nyɛ, nɩ a ala fʋn wõ.
44022016	Pʋ̃pãanyã, bo lɛ fʋ lɛ chɛlɛ go? Ir a ba so fʋ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ka a na pɛɛ a fʋ yeldɛbɛ bar a fʋ bʋɔlɔ a sɩ Soro yuor.'
44022017	"A lɛ ɩn lɩɛb wa a Jerusalɛm naa tɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn be a puorfʋ yir, ka a wa kaara ma jãna kaar.
44022018	Ka n nyɛ a sɩ Soro na 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr kʋrɔ ma. Wʋ 'yɛr naa, 'Pɔɔ fɔɔ na fʋ yi ka a Jerusalɛm ajienaa, bojũu nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ sɔɔ a lɛ fʋn na 'yɛr a n 'yɛr ɛ.'
44022019	Ka n 'yɛr sɔɔ wʋ, 'N Soro a nɩbɛ banyãna bɔ̃ɔn naa a lɛ ɩn yʋɔrɔ a lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir naa nyɔɔrɔ ba pɔɔrɔ tɩ ŋmiere a bala na sɔɔ de fʋ.
44022020	A daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ban kʋrɔ a fʋ dãasɩ dire Sɩteven maa nɩ bala jaa ɩn nɛbʋ̃'yen ka n kaara a ba fuusɩ tɩ ba kʋ wʋ.'
44022021	Ka a sɩ Soro pãa 'yɛr kʋ ma, 'Chen, ɩn tʋ̃ fʋn tɛɛr jaa be a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ pɔ.' "
44022022	A nɩyɔɔ bala chɛlɛ naa lɛ a Pɔɔl na 'yɛrɛ wa tãn a jie wʋn 'yɛr a nɩyor pɔ chenfʋ 'yɛr, a ba pãa tãna 'yɛrɛ, "Yɩ ŋmaa wʋ ju, a ba sɛɛ ɩka wʋ lɛ chɛnɛ vʋrɔ ɛ."
44022023	Lɛ lɛ ba pɔɔrɔ a gɔ̃mɔ̃ tɩ lɔɔrɔ a ba fɔɔr ɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a tãna lɔɔrɔ a saaju.
44022024	Ka a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ vɛ̃ ka ba tara a Pɔɔl kpɛ̃n be a sojasɩ yir. Wʋ 'yɛr ɩka ba fɔb a Pɔɔl a wʋ wiil ba bãa lɛ so a nɩbɛ pɔɔrɔ a gɔ̃mɔ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ a lɛ.
44022025	A lɛ ban lũ a Pɔɔl ɩka ba fɔb, ka wʋ sʋʋr a sojasɩ nɩdier na ara a be, "A tara na sɔr ka yɩn fɔb a Worom nɩrɛ na yaa sʋʋr kaa a yelnyɩnɛ wʋn ɩ ɛ?"
44022026	Lɛ a sojasɩ nɩdier na wa wõ a nɩtɔ̃ wʋ chen a ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr, "Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ fʋn ɩ? A daba nyã ɩn Worom nɩrɛ."
44022027	Ka a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ chen a Pɔɔl sɛ̃ tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "'Yɛr kʋ ma, Worom nɩrɛ lɛ fʋ ɩ ɔ?" Ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr ɩka, "Ɔ̃ɔ."
44022028	A sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ pãa 'yɛr, "Maa 'lɔ, libiyɔɔ lɛ n yab tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a ka." Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "Maa 'lɔ, ka lɛ ba dɔɔ ma."
44022029	Ka a bala na ara gu a wʋ fɔbfʋ mɩ tɔɔ yaar ajienaa. Dãbɩ̃ɛ mɩ kpɛ̃n a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a lɛ wʋn wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Pɔɔl ɩn Worom nɩrɛ tɩchɛ ka wʋ vɛ̃ a ba lũ wʋ.
44022030	A wɛr na wa chaar, a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔ bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ ba bara a Pɔɔl ɛ. Wʋ for wʋn bar tɩ bʋɔl a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ nɩbɛrɛ ka ba jaa lɔ̃ɔ taa. Tɩ wʋ pãa suu waan a Pɔɔl a wʋ wa ara a ba niem.
44023001	Pɔɔl kãan a nɩbɛrɛ a lɛ a dẽdẽe tɩ 'yɛr, "N yɛɛr, n tʋ̃n a lɛ na sɛɛ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn wa ta a dɩna tɩ n nyãa ba dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ."
44023002	A anyãna wʋn 'yɛr ka a Ananias na ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr kʋ a bala na ara gbʋr a Pɔɔl ɩka ba 'ma wʋ a nɛɛ pɔ.
44023003	Ka a Pɔɔl pãa 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Nãaŋmɩn na 'ma fʋ naa a fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ a tãpɩɛl dachin nyã. Fʋ jɛ̃n a be ɩka fʋ tɔɔr a n 'yɛr a lɛ a nɛɛ na bin tɩ na fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ lɛ sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nɛɛ, na fʋ 'yɛr ɩka ba 'ma ma."
44023004	A bala na ara gbʋr a Pɔɔl 'yɛr kʋ, "Aa! Bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ fʋ tʋrɔ ɔ?"
44023005	Ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "Yɛɛr n ba bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ ɛ, bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, 'Taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɛrɛ 'yɛrdɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ nɩbɛ nɩdier ɛ.' "
44023006	Pɔɔl na wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Saduseemɩne jɛr naa Faraseemɩne pɔ ka wʋ tãn kpɛ̃ɔ jaa be a nɩbɛrɛ pɔ na wʋ 'yɛr, "N yɛɛr, Farasee lɛ n ɩ, ka a Farasee nɩrɛ dɔɔ ma. N ara naa kana a ban tɔɔr a n 'yɛr, bojũu n sɔɔ naa ɩka kũu pɔ irfʋ ben be."
44023007	A lɛ wʋn wa 'yɛr a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ ka a nɛchɩrɛ lo a Faraseemɩne nɩ a Saduseemɩne chara pɔ, ka a lɔ̃ɔfʋ ŋma jiir ayi.
44023008	Saduseemɩne 'yɛr ɩka kũu pɔ irfʋ ba be be ɛ, malakasɩ nɩ a nɩsɩɩr mɩ ba be be ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a Faraseemɩne 'lɔ sɔɔn ɩka a jaa ben be.
44023009	A gɔ̃mɔ̃ pɔɔfʋ tɩ gar naa ka a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wiwiilbe bamɩne na ɩ a Faraseemɩne ir ara tɩ chɩɩr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa ɩka, "Sɩn 'lɔ ba nyɛ a daba nyã chɛfʋ jie ɛ, tɩ ala wa ɩ sɩɛ kɔ̃ɔ bɩɩ malaka lɛ 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ wʋ?"
44023010	A nɛchɩrɛ wa tɩ gar naa, ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a wʋ man tãa ban wa tɔɔr a Pɔɔl 'mɛl, ala lɛ so ka wʋ vɛ̃ a sojasɩ suu tɩ faa a Pɔɔl don be a sojasɩ yir.
44023011	A tɩ̃sɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, a sɩ Soro wa ara na gbʋr a Pɔɔl tɩ 'yɛr, "Nyɔɔ nyãa, a lɛ fʋn man a n yelmɩ̃ɛ a ka a Jerusalɛm mɩ tɩ man a lɛ nɛ a be a Worom tẽe pɔ."
44023012	Wɛr na wa chaar bibio, a Juu nɩbɛ bamɩne jɛ̃n guor taa na ba pɔ'yɔ̃ɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛrɛ ɩka ba kʋ̃ di bon jaa ɛ, bɩɩ nyũ bon jaa ɛ, ka bala baa kʋ a Pɔɔl ɛ.
44023013	Ba gar dɔɔr lɩjaayi na guor a guorfʋ nyãna.
44023014	Ba chen a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃, na ba tɩ 'yɛr, "Sɩ bin nɛɛ ɩka sɩ kʋ̃ di bon jaa ɛ, ka sɩn baa kʋ a Pɔɔl baar ɛ.
44023015	Pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩn nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ nɩbɛrɛ yɩ tʋ̃ 'yɛr a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a wʋ waan a Pɔɔl a yɩ sʋʋr yele kɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a par. Sɩn na var gu be a sɔr pɔ kʋ wʋ ka waa ta a be a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ."
44023016	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl arbile wõ a guorfʋ nyã na wʋ chen be a sojasɩ yir na wʋ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a Pɔɔl.
44023017	Ka a Pɔɔl bʋɔl a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Tara a pɔlbile nyãna chiin a yɩ jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sɛ̃ wʋ tara na 'yɛr na 'yɛr kʋ wʋ."
44023018	Lɛ lɛ wʋ tara a pɔlbile chiin a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sɛ̃ na wʋ tɩ 'yɛr, "A Pɔɔl na be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ lɛ tʋ̃ bʋɔl ma na wʋ 'yɛr ɩka n tara a pɔlbile nyãna waan a fʋ sɛ̃, ka wʋ tara na 'yɛr na 'yɛr kʋ fʋ."
44023019	Ka a sojasɩ ba jaa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyɔɔ a pɔlbile nũu tɔɔ yin chɛ̃chɛ̃ɛ tɩ sʋʋr wʋ, "Baa lɛ fʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka fʋ 'yɛr kʋ ma?"
44023020	A wʋ 'yɛr, "A Juu nɩbɛ guor taa na ban sʋɔr fʋ ka fʋn waan a Pɔɔl a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ sɛ̃ a bio ka a kaara fɩka ba bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba sʋʋr wʋ yele kɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a par.
44023021	Ta sɔɔ ɛ, bojũu ba gar nɩbɛ lɩjaayi na var gu wʋ, ba pɔn 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ ɩka ba kʋ̃ di bon ɛ, bɩɩ nyũ bon jaa ɛ, ka bala ba kʋ wʋ ɛ. Bala ben chɔɔr baar a pʋ̃pãanyã tɩ chɛlɛ a fʋ nɛɛ."
44023022	Ka a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ bar a pɔlbile sɔr tɩ kpãa wʋ 'yɛr, "Taa ɩrɛ wa vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka fʋ wan a n sɛ̃ ɛ."
44023023	Tɩ pãa bʋɔl a wʋ nɩbɛrɛ ayi na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ chɔɔr sojasɩ kɔɔr ayi (200) na yɩ lɛ chɔɔr a sojasɩ lɩjaata nɩ pie (70) na bɔ̃ɔ wiisɩ dofʋ, nɩ sojasɩ kɔɔr ayi (200) mɩ na bɔ̃ɔ a pɩ̃ɩ woor ala lɔbfʋ ka yɩ chen a Sisariya a tɩ̃sɔɔ nyãna.
44023024	Yɩ bɔ a wii ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋ a Pɔɔl a wʋ do jɩ̃nɛ a yɩ chiin wʋ vɩla tɩ kʋ a paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ Feliksɩ."
44023025	A gãn wʋn sɛb 'lɔ nɩ nyã,
44023026	"Maa Kɩlaudiyus Lisiyasɩ lɛ sɛɛrɛ a gãn nyãna kʋrɔ a fʋ̃ʋ Feliksɩ a paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ naa, n puor fʋ naa.
44023027	A daba nyãna lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ nyɔɔ na ba ta ɩka ba kʋ, tɩchɛ ɩn wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Worom nɩrɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ, n chiin naa a n sojasɩ tɩ faan wʋ.
44023028	N ta bʋɔrɔ na ɩka n bɔ̃ɔ a yele 'lɔ jũu ban ba bara wʋ ɛ, naa de wʋ chiin be a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ nɩbɛrɛ sɛ̃.
44023029	Naa tɩ nyɛ ka ɩ a yele ɩ naa a ba nɛbinãa yele lɛ. Tɩchɛ saa lɛ nyɛ yele jaa wʋn maal na wʋ sɛɛn kũu bɩɩ die pɔ pɔɔfʋ ɛ.
44023030	Lɛ ban wa man kʋ ma ban guoro a daba nyã yele, ala lɛ so ka n vɛ̃ ka ba tara wʋ a fɔɔ a lɛ nɛ waan a fʋ sɛ̃. N mɩ 'yɛr kʋ a bala na tuoro wʋ a yele ɩka ba wa a fʋ sɛ̃ wa 'yɛr a fʋ mɩ kaa."
44023031	A sojasɩ tun a lɛ a ba nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na 'yɛr na ba de a Pɔɔl a tɩ̃sɔɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ jaa na ba tɩ tãn Antɩpatɩrsɩ tẽe pɔ.
44023032	Wɛr na wa chaar, ba vɛ̃n ka a wiir dẽme tara a Pɔɔl chiine, tɩchɛ ka a gbɛɛ dẽme lɩɛb wa a sojasɩ yir.
44023033	Lɛ ban tɩ ta a Sisariya tẽe pɔ ba den a gãn na ba kʋ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ tɩ de a Pɔɔl mɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ nũu pɔ.
44023034	Ka a paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kar a gãn tɩ na wʋ sʋʋr a Pɔɔl a tẽbuor wʋn yi, wʋn wa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Sɩlɩsɩya lɛ wʋ yi.
44023035	Ka a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛr, "A bala na tuo fʋ a yele wa ta ala lɛ ɩn wõ a fʋ 'yɛr." Wʋ vɛ̃n ka ba tara a Pɔɔl kpɛ̃n be a yir kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ pɔ a Nãa Hɛrɔd na dɔ̃ɔ mɛ tɩ guro wʋ.
44024001	A ber anũu puor lɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ Ananias suun chen be a Sisariya nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ bamɩne, ka a Tɛtulusɩ na ɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ pʋɔ ba a ba 'mataa chen na tɩ 'yɛr a Pɔɔl 'yɛr a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ niem.
44024002	Ban bʋɔl a Pɔɔl kpɛ̃n ka a Tɛtulusɩ na man a wʋ yele kʋ a Feliksɩ na wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Sɩ din nʋ̃ɔ kor a fʋ jũu, ka a fʋ yɛ̃ lɩɛr yelvɩɛlsɩ kʋ a fʋ paal.
44024003	Jie jaa nɩ sɔr jaa pɔ fʋ ɩn nɩkpɛ̃vɩla, a sɩ sɔɔ de fʋ nɩ nuur ayi nɩ pʋpɛl.
44024004	Tɩchɛ n ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka n dam fʋ yɔɔ ɛ, yelbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ n bʋɔrɔ ɩka n sʋɔr jaa bɩ̃lãa ka fʋ di kãnyir kʋ sɩ.
44024005	Sɩ nyɛn a daba nyãna ka wʋ ɩ gɔ̃bʋɔrɔ, a Juu nɩbɛ ba jaa lɛ wʋ ma tɔ a ba jur gbõtaa a wɛr wʋ jaa, na wʋ ɩ a nɩbɛ bala na turo a Najaretɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ nɩdiere.
44024006	Na wʋ bʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir sɔ̃ɔ barfʋ, ala lɛ so ka sɩ nyɔɔ wʋ.
44024008	Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ fʋ sʋʋr wʋ kaa fʋn nyɛn bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a ala sɩn 'yɛrɛ dɔɔlɔ wʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ."
44024009	Ka a Juu nɩbɛ ba jaa na be be 'yɛr ɩka a lɛ a Tɛtulusɩ na 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ.
44024010	A paal nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kʋn a Pɔɔl sɔr a wʋ 'yɛr, ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "N bɔ̃ɔn naa an ɩ yuom yɔɔ lɛ fʋ kaa a paal nyãna, a nʋ̃mɔ̃ ma naa ka n na 'yɛr a n 'yɛr.
44024011	Fʋ̃ʋ sʋʋr ban 'yɛr ɩka a ba gar ber pie nɩ ayi ɩn chen be a Jerusalɛm ɩka n tɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn ɛ.
44024012	Ba ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba nyɛ ma ka n chɩrɛ nɩ nɩrɛ jaa be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ɛ, bɩɩ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩyɔɔ be a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir ɛ, bɩɩ a tẽe pɔ jie jaa ɛ.
44024013	A anyãna ban 'yɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ wiil ma a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
44024014	Tɩchɛ n sɔɔ naa ɩka n puoro naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne na dɔ̃ɔ puoro naa lɛ turo a Sɔr 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a sɔr yuo. N sɔɔn de a ala a jaa, na a sɔɔ lɛ a nɛɛ na sɔɔ nɩ a ala a jaa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb.
44024015	N mɩ tara naa a tɩɛrtɔ bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩtãa a ba kaar ɩka nɩsʋ̃n nɩ a putudẽme na ir ɩ vʋɛ.
44024016	Ala lɛ so ka n mʋɔrɔ sɔ̃ɔ jaa ɩka a n pʋtɩɛr wʋ chaar Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a nɩrɛ niem.
44024017	"N yin kor, tɩ naa lɛ lɩɛb wa a Jerusalɛm nɩ libie ɩka n wa kʋ a nɔ̃n dẽme tɩ naa mɩ lo bɔɔr kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn.
44024018	N dɔ̃ɔ pɔl a n mɩ̃ɛ baar a lɛ ban nyɛ ma a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ. Nɩyɔɔ ba dɔ̃ɔ pʋɔ ma ɛ, n mɩ ba dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ damfʋ jaa ɛ.
44024019	Tɩchɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi a Asɩya paal pɔ wa, bala mɩ lɛ a ta sɛɛ ɩka ba be ka na ba 'yɛr a n 'yɛr.
44024020	Bɩɩ a banyãna na be ka a ba wiil a yelnyɩnɛ ban nyɛ ɩn maal, a lɛ ɩn ara a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ niem.
44024021	Ala ba ɩ a 'yɛr bir bʋ̃'yen nyãna tɛɛ ɩn 'yɛr kpɛ̃ɔ jaa a lɛ ɩn ara a ba niem naa 'yɛr, 'A kũn na ir ɩ vʋɛ, naa be ara a yɩ niem a yɩn tɔɔr a n 'yɛr a dɩna.' "
44024022	A Feliksɩ na wa pãa bɔ̃ɔn a Sɔr yele wʋ wɛl a nɩbɛ bar tɩ 'yɛr, "A Lisiyasɩ na ɩ a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ wa wa ala lɛ ɩn 'yɛr a fʋ 'yɛr."
44024023	Wʋ den a Pɔɔl kʋ a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ tɩ 'yɛr ɩka a wʋ ma kʋ wʋ sɔr tɩ sɔɔ ka a Pɔɔl barmɩne ma sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ nɩ a wʋ bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ.
44024024	A maal ber aŋmɩnɛ jaa tɩchɛ ka a Feliksɩ tara a wʋ pɔɔ Durusila na ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ waan. Wʋ tʋ̃n ka ba waan a Pɔɔl a wʋ chɛlɛ a lɛ wʋn mana a lɛ fʋn na sɔɔ de a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto.
44024025	Pɔɔl 'yɛr naa a lɛ nɛ wa pʋr yeltorsɩ yuor nɩ mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔfʋ nɩ lɛ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ na waara. Ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a Feliksɩ a wʋ 'yɛr, "Pʋ̃pãanyã a sɛɛn lɛ, chiine maa wa tara jaa ɩn tʋ̃n bʋɔl fʋ."
44024026	Wʋ tɩɛr man taa Pɔɔl na kʋ wʋn libie, na wʋ ma bʋɔlɔ a Pɔɔl jaa tɔ̃tɔ̃ ma 'yɛrɛ nɩ wʋ.
44024027	Yuom ayi na wa po Pɔsɩyusɩ Festus den a Feliksɩ jie, tɩchɛ a Feliksɩ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ pɛl a Juu nɩbɛ pʋɔ jũu, wʋ bar a Pɔɔl a be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ.
44025001	Festus na de a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ maal ber ata wʋ yin be a Sisariya chen a Jerusalɛm.
44025002	Be lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a ba nɩdierbe man a 'yɛr ala ban tara nɩ, a Pɔɔl kʋ wʋ.
44025003	Ba sʋɔr a Festus nɩbijɩɛ jaa ɩka a lɛ ban sʋɔrɔ wʋ a wʋ sɔɔ na wʋ vɛ̃ a ba tara a Pɔɔl waan be a Jerusalɛm an ɩ ba chɔɔr ũu gu na kʋ a Pɔɔl a be a sɔr pɔ.
44025004	Ka a Festus 'yɛr, "A Pɔɔl ben a be a Sisariya a maa mɩ̃ɛ a kʋ̃ kor ɛ, tɩchɛ ka n chen a be.
44025005	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ nɩbɛrɛ bamɩne pʋɔ ma a sɩ 'mataa chen, ala ɩ wʋ maal yeldɛɛr a yɩ 'yɛr n kaa."
44025006	Wʋn wa maal a be ber aniin bɩɩ pie wʋ chen a Sisariya, wʋn tɩ gã ir wʋ jɩ̃nɛ naa a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr ɩka ba waan a Pɔɔl.
44025007	Ban wa waan a Pɔɔl a Juu nɩbɛ bala na yi a Jerusalɛm wa ara na jilʋ̃ wʋ ŋmara jir kara dɔɔlɔ wʋ tɩchɛ ba maa tʋ̃ɔ wiil a par ɛ.
44025008	A Pɔɔl pãa 'yɛr, "Maa ba maal dɛɛr jaa ɛ, naa sɔ̃ɔ a Juu nɩbɛ nɛbinãa nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ɛ, bɩɩ 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa ɛ."
44025009	Festus bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ pɛl a Juu nɩbɛ pʋɔ na wʋ sʋʋr a Pɔɔl, "Fʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka fʋ do a Jerusalɛm ka a 'yɛr anyãna ban 'yɛr dɔɔl fʋ ka n tɩ tɔɔr a be bɩɩ?"
44025010	A Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "Pʋ̃pãanyã, n ben ara a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie a be an sɛɛ ɩka ba tɔɔr a n 'yɛr. N mɩ ba maal yeldɛɛr jaa a Juu nɩbɛ sɛ̃ ɛ, a lɛ a fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ na bɔ̃ɔn.
44025011	Maa ta maal dɛɛr naa sɛɛn kũu n kʋ̃ naa tɔr ɩka n kpi ɛ. Tɩchɛ a 'yɛr anyãna a Juu nɩbɛ na 'yɛr dɔɔl ma na ba ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa ba tara sɔr na fɩr ma kʋ ba ɛ. Siisa sɛ̃ lɛ ɩn chen ka wʋ tɩ tɔɔr a n 'yɛr."
44025012	Lɛ a Festus nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛrɛ na wa man taa baar wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Pɔɔl, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ sʋɔr ɩka a Siisa sɛ̃ lɛ fʋn chen, be lɛ fʋn chen."
44025013	A kor bɩ̃lãa ka a Nãa Agripa nɩ a wʋ yɛpɔɔ Bernisɩ wa be a Sisariya ɩka ba wa puor a Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ Festus.
44025014	An ɩ ban jɛ̃n a be kor jũu, Festus mana naa a Pɔɔl yele kʋrɔ a Nãa Agripa 'yɛrɛ, "Daba kɔ̃ɔ lɛ be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ a Feliksɩ na pɔɔ.
44025015	A lɛ ɩn chen a Jerusalɛm, a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a ba nɩdierbe den yelyɔɔ dɔɔl wʋ na ba sʋɔr ma ɩka n tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr ge wʋ.
44025016	"Ka n 'yɛr kʋ ba a Worom nɩbɛ maa tɔɔr nɩrɛ 'yɛr ala ɩ a nɩnyɩnɛ ban 'yɛr a 'yɛr dɔɔl ba wa ara a bala na tara nɩ wʋ a 'yɛr niem na wʋ 'yɛr a wʋ nɛɛ 'yɛr ɛ.
44025017	Ala lɛ so ka ba pɔɔ ma a sɩ 'mataa wa a ka, n ba wa jɛ̃n a 'yɛr ɛ, a wɛr na wa chaar n jɛ̃ naa na tɔɔr a 'yɛr naa vɛ̃ ka ba waan a daba.
44025018	A bala na tara nɩ wʋ a 'yɛr na wa ir ara na 'yɛr, baa 'yɛr 'yɛr jaa na ɩ dɛɛr nɩtãa lɛ ɩn tɩɛr ban taa 'yɛr ɛ.
44025019	Tɩchɛ a ba 'yɛr tɩ ɩ naa a ba puorfʋ yele lɛ nɩ daba kɔ̃ɔ na di Yesu na kpi ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr ɩka wʋ ir naa na wʋ ɩ vʋr.
44025020	Ka a yele nyã sɔb ma nɩbir, n ba bɔ̃ɔ ŋmɩnɛ ɩn na ɩ vɩɛr a yele nyã ɛ, ala lɛ so ka n sʋʋr wʋ ala ɩ wʋn bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ chen a Jerusalɛm ka ba tɩ tɔɔr a 'yɛr anyãna a be.
44025021	Pɔɔl 'lɔ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa wʋ tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr, n vɛ̃n a ba tara wʋ tɩ tãn a lɛ ɩn na bar sɔr ka ba tara wʋ chiin a Siisa sɛ̃."
44025022	Ka a Nãa Agripa pãa 'yɛr kʋ a Festus, "Maa mɩ̃ɛ naa bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n wõ a daba mɩ kɔkɔr." Ka a Festus 'yɛr, "Bio fʋn wõn a wʋ kɔkɔr."
44025023	A wɛr na wa chaar, a Nãa Agripa nɩ a Bernisɩ wa naa ka a nɩbɛ de 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋ ba ka ba tɩ kpɛ̃n be a dikpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ pɔ ban ma lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a sojasɩ nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a tẽe nɩbɛrɛ. Ka a Festus vɛ̃ a sojasɩ tara a Pɔɔl waan.
44025024	Ka a Festus 'yɛr, "Nãa Agripa nɩ a yɩn bala jaa na be ka a sɩ sɛ̃, yɩ nyɛ a daba nyãna, a Juu nɩbɛ ba jaa 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ma be a Jerusalɛm nɩ a ka a Sisariya tãna 'yɛrɛ ɩka a ba sɛɛ ka wʋ lɛ chɛnɛ go ɛ.
44025025	N mɩ ba nyɛ yele jaa wʋn ɩ ka a tara sɔr ka sɩn kʋ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ bojũu wʋ sʋɔr sɔr ɩka wʋ chen a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa sɛ̃, n mɩ na bar wʋn sɔr ka wʋ chen a Worom.
44025026	Tɩchɛ n ba tara a wʋ yele ala na sɛɛ ka n na sɛb kʋ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ ɛ. A lɛ jũu n waan wʋ naa a yɩ jaa niem nɩ a fʋ̃ʋ Nãa Agripa niem a fʋ mɩ jʋʋr a wʋ yele kaa, ka n bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ ɩn na sɛb.
44025027	Bojũu, a ba sɛɛn ma ɛ, ka n na vɛ̃ ka ba tara nɩrɛ ban pɔɔ chiine naa ba wiil a yelnyɩnɛ wʋn maal ɛ."
44026001	Kaa Agripa pãa 'yɛr kʋ a Pɔɔl, "Fʋ tara na sɔr na 'yɛr a fʋ nɛɛ 'yɛr." Pɔɔl tur naa a nũu tɩ piel mana a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yele,
44026002	"Nãa Agripa, a ɩ man bɔɔsʋ̃n ɩn ara a fʋ niem a dɩna naa na man a n yele ala a jaa a Juu nɩbɛ na 'yɛr dɔɔl ma.
44026003	Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ, a fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa a Juu nɩbɛ yelbinsɩ a jaa nɩ a ba nɛchɩrɛ, a lɛ jũu n sʋɔr fʋ naa ka fʋ di kãnyir chɛlɛ ma.
44026004	"A Juu nɩbɛ ba jaa bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ ɩn be a bibile daar jaa, a maa paal pɔ nɩ a ka a Jerusalɛm mɩ.
44026005	Ba bɔ̃ɔ man kor na ban tʋ̃ɔ di a lɛ dãasɩɛ ala ɩ ba bʋɔrɔ naa. Ba bɔ̃ɔn ma naa ɩn turo yele jaa nɛ nɛ nɛ a sɩ puorfʋ pɔ, naa ɩ a Farasee nɩrɛ.
44026006	A pʋ̃pãanyã a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a sɩ sãakpãmɩne ka n tara a tɩɛr jũu lɛ so ka n 'yɛr be tɔɔrɔ a dɩna.
44026007	A nɛ tɩra anyãna jũu lɛ a sɩn bʋrɔ pie nɩ ayi ɩ a sɩ tɩɛrtɔ fʋ jie, ka a na wa ɩ a sɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir puoro a Nãaŋmɩn mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ. A fʋ̃ʋ nãa a tɩɛrtɔ nyãna jũu, a Juu nɩbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma a 'yɛr.
44026008	Bo lɛ so ka yɩ tɩɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɩ̃ɩ kũu ɛ?
44026009	"A maa mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ŋme nyãa naa ɩka ɩn ɩ naa lɛ jaa ɩn na tʋ̃ɔ naa sɔ̃ɔ a Yesu na yi a Najaretɩ yuor.
44026010	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ n ɩ be a Jerusalɛm. A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ kʋ man sɔr ka n nyɔɔr a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo yɔɔ naa pɔɔ, bala wa kʋrɔ ba n ma sɔɔ naa.
44026011	Sɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ jaa, n ma chen a be a ba lɔ̃ɔfʋ jiir naa tɩ ge ge ba, naa ma fɩrɛ ba 'yɛr 'yɛr dɛbɛ tɩchɛ a maa tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a lɛ ɛ. A lɛ a ba yele na dire ma a suur n ma chen a wɛr yuo pɔ tɩ ge ba a be.
44026012	"Ala jũu lɛ a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ dɔ̃ɔ kʋ ma a sɔr ka n chiine a Damaskus.
44026013	Mɔ̃tɔ̃tuo sɔ̃ɔ lɛ fʋ̃ʋ nãa, a lɛ ɩn be a sɔr pɔ, n nyɛn chãa na yi saaju chaar mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na wʋ jilʋ̃ ma nɩ a bala ɩn lɔ̃ɔ chiine.
44026014	Sɩ jaa lon tẽe tɩchɛ ka n wõ nɩrɛ na sʋrɔ ma nɩ a Heburu kɔkɔr, 'Sɔɔl, Sɔɔl bo lɛ fʋ gere ma a lɛ? Fʋ wõn tuo fʋn tɛb a dakʋra.'
44026015	Be lɛ n pãa sʋʋr, 'Fʋ̃ʋ nɩ ana, Soro?' A wʋ 'yɛr, 'Maa lɛ a Yesu 'lɔ fʋn gere.
44026016	Pʋ̃pãanyã ir ara, n yi fʋ naa, naa ir fʋ a fʋn ɩ a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ na fʋ mʋɔlɔ a ala fʋn nyɛ a dɩna nɩ a ala ɩn na wiil fʋ.
44026017	Ɩn faa fʋ naa a fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ nuur pɔ, nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ nuur pɔ. Maa lɛ tʋ̃nɔ̃ fʋ,
44026018	tɩ yuo a ba nɩbie na fʋ tɔɔ ba yin a libe pɔ, waan a chãa pɔ, na fʋ yin a Satan kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ, waan a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, a wʋ vɛ̃ a ba yelbier kʋ ba ka ba mɩ nyɛ jie nɩ a bala na sɔɔ de ma, ka n faa ba.'
44026019	"A lɛ jũu, Nãa Agripa, n ba tɔr a nyɛfʋ nyã na yi a saaju ɛ.
44026020	N den nie man kʋ a Damaskus dẽme, nɩ a Jerusalɛm dẽme, nɩ a Judiya wɛr wʋ jaa, nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ mɩ. N mʋɔl kʋ ba ɩka ba lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr, na ba lɩɛb wa Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, na ba vɛ̃ ka ba tʋ̃mɔ̃ wiil ɩka ba lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr.
44026021	Ala lɛ so a Juu nɩbɛ nyɔɔ ma a ba puorfʋ yir bɛchaar pɔ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba kʋ ma.
44026022	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ sʋ̃ʋ ma wa tãn a dɩna, ka n be ara na man kʋ nɩrɛ jaa. N ba 'yɛr 'yɛr jaa tɩ põn a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ na 'yɛr ɩka an ɩ naa ɛ,
44026023	ɩka a Nɩ-iraa na din dɔɔyɛ na wʋ mɩ ɩ nɩrɛ na de nie ir a kũu pɔ, na wʋ man a chãa 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ."
44026024	Kana lɛ a Pɔɔl ta ka a Festus kpɛ tãn wʋ tɩ 'yɛr, "Pɔɔl a tɩɛr bɔr fʋ naa, a jãn yɔɔ vɛ̃n ka fʋ gele."
44026025	Ka a Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ Festus n ba gele ɛ, ala ɩn 'yɛrɛ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ yɛ̃ 'yɛr.
44026026	A nãa bɔ̃ɔn a yele anyãna ala lɛ so ka n lɔb yãan bar tɩ 'yɛrɛ nɩ wʋ. N sɔɔ naa ɩka a yele anyãna ba sɔɔl wʋ ɛ, bojũu a yele nyã ba ɩ libe pɔ ɛ.
44026027	Nãa Agripa, fʋ sɔɔn a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ bɩɩ? N bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka fʋ sɔɔ naa."
44026028	Ka a Nãa Agripa pãa sʋʋr a Pɔɔl, "Fʋ tɩɛr man tãa a dɩna tɛɛ lɛ fʋn lɩɛb ma ka n ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto turo bɩɩ?"
44026029	A Pɔɔl 'yɛr, "Ka dɩna tɛɛ lɛ bɩɩ daar kɔ̃ɔ lɛ yo, n sʋɔrɔ naa Nãaŋmɩn ɩka a ta ɩ a fʋ̃ʋ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩ nɩrɛ jaa na chɛlɛ a 'yɛr nyãna a dɩna ka yɩ kaara a n kaar tɩ na ba taa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ yɩ a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ anyãna ɛ."
44026030	Ka a nãa vaa ir nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a Bernisɩ lɔ̃ɔn a bala wʋn 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ nɩ.
44026031	Ba yin a die pɔ, pãa 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr kʋrɔ taa na ba 'yɛrɛ, "A daba nyãna ba maal yele jaa na sɛɛn kũu bɩɩ pɔɔfʋ ɛ."
44026032	Ka a Agripa 'yɛr kʋ a Festus, "Fʋn taa tʋ̃ɔ bar a daba nyãna ala ɩ waa ta sʋɔr sɔr ɩka wʋn chen a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa sɛ̃ ɛ."
44027001	An wa ta ɩka sɩn chen a Itali, ba den a Pɔɔl nɩ a bamɩne ban pɔɔ kʋ a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ban bʋɔlɔ Julius, wʋ ɩ naa a nãkpɛ̃ɛ soja kpɛ̃ɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ.
44027002	Sɩ kpɛ̃n a gboro kpɛ̃ɛ na yi a Adɩramatiyum ka wʋ ir an ɩ Asɩya kõkoor lɛ wʋn lana. Aristakus na ɩ a Masedonɩya paal nɩrɛ na wʋ yi a Tɛsalonika pʋɔ sɩ naa.
44027003	A wɛr na wa chaar, sɩ tãn a Sidon tẽe pɔ, ka a Julius maal a Pɔɔl vɩla na wʋ bar wʋ sɔr ka wʋ chen a wʋ barmɩne sɛ̃ ka ba tɩ sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ.
44027004	Be lɛ sɩ lɛ yin a gboro lana a Sipurusɩ bojũu a sɛsɛbɛ furo na tuoro sɩ.
44027005	A lɛ sɩn wa gɔ̃ɔ a man sãlsɔɔ Sɩlɩsɩya nɩ a Pamfiliya kõkoor lɛ sɩ wa ara nɩ a Mira na be a Lisiya wɛr pɔ.
44027006	Be lɛ a soja nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyɛ a Aleksandiriya gboro kpɛ̃ɛ na chiine a Itali ka wʋ wɛl sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
44027007	A ber waa naa sɩn maal a sɔr pɔ, jaa vɛ̃ nɛ nɛ nɛ lɛ sɩ chiine ka a wõ sɩ tɩ sɩ tɩ ta a Sɩnidusɩ tẽe pɔ. Lɛ a sɛsɛbɛ na ba sɔɔrɔ a sɩ chiine a dẽdẽe ɛ, a gboro tun sɩ naa a Kɩrete a Salmone tẽe puor.
44027008	A man kõkoor lɛ sɩ lana ka a wõ sɩ tɩ tãn a jie ban bʋɔlɔ a Gboro Juvɩla Ara A Jie na gbʋr a Lasea tẽe.
44027009	Sɩ sɔ̃ɔn sɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ a sɔr pɔ a sɛsɛbɛ na furo jũu, ka a gboro chenfʋ mɩ kʋrɔ dãbɩ̃ɛ bojũu Kɔ̃ Galfʋ sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ mɩ po naa, ka a Pɔɔl kpãana ba 'yɛrɛ,
44027010	"Nɩbɛ, n kãan nyɛ ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ be a sɩ chenfʋ pɔ, yelyɔɔ na sɔ̃ɔ naa, a gboro tuor nɩ a sɩn mɩ̃ɛ mɩ."
44027011	Tɩchɛ a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ba chɛlɛ a lɛ a Pɔɔl na 'yɛrɛ ɛ, tɩ sɔɔ a lɛ a gboro mɔ̃nɔ̃ nɩ lɛ a gboro sʋɔ na 'yɛr.
44027012	A gboro ara a jie ba sɛɛn ban na ara a be a ɔɔr sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a ba yɔɔ jaa 'yɛr naa ɩka ba po chiine, tɩɛrɛ ɩka ban tãn a Fonɩksɩ na ba ara a be. A Kɩrete gboro ara a jie lɛ na tor a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie guba nɩ a nũsʋ̃ɔ jie.
44027013	Lɛ a sɛsɛbaalʋ̃ʋ na wa furo yire a guba jie, ba tɩɛr ɩka ba nyɛn a lɛ ban bʋɔrɔ, ba for a kur nɛbie bara tɩ lana nɩ a gboro a Kɩrete gogoro.
44027014	An wa kor bɩ̃lãa, ka a sɛsɛbɛ kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie guba sɛsɛbɛ fun yi a be wa.
44027015	A sɛsɛbɛ tʋ̃ɔn a gboro a waa lɛ tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ chiine a niem ɛ, ka a sɛsɛbɛ pãa tara sɩ chiine.
44027016	A lɛ sɩn wa pɩ̃ a dõdolbile ɩ̃sʋɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Kawuda, a ɩn tuo kʋ sɩ ka sɩn 'mɔɔ a gborbile.
44027017	Lɛ a nɩbɛ na wa 'mɔɔ a gborbile ka wʋ do, ba den miir lũ gbɛb a gborkpɛ̃ɛ. Sɩ joro na dãbɩ̃ɛ ɩka sɩ taa ɩrɛ wa tɩ mʋr a Sirtisɩ bire pɔ ɛ, ka ba bar a kur nɛbie ka a gboro pãa tɔɔrɔ.
44027018	A sɛsɛkpɛ̃ɛ nyã mɔ̃n sɩn jaa ka wɛr wa chaar ka ba piel wɛlɛ a tuor lɔɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ.
44027019	A ber ata daar a gboro dẽme mɩ̃ɛ foro naa a gboro bomo nɩ a ba mɩ̃ɛ nuur lɔɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ.
44027020	Lɛ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ a ŋmarbie na ba lɛ wa nyɩr ɛ, a ber waa naa tɩchɛ ka a sɛkpɛ̃ɛ chɛnɛ ire ka a sɩ chɩ̃ɛfʋ tɩɛrtɔ jie baar.
44027021	A ber wa po naa tɩ baa di bon jaa ɛ, ka a Pɔɔl ir ara a ba sãlsɔɔ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Nɩbɛ, yɩn ta sɔɔ tu a n nɛɛ ka sɩ ta chɛnɛ be a be Kɩrete a wõm nyãna kʋ̃ naa pɔɔ sɩ ɛ, ka a bonsɩ be wɛ ɛ.
44027022	Tɩchɛ n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa, yɩ nyɔɔ nyãa bojũu ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ bɔr ɛ, a gboro tɛɛ lɛ na wɛ.
44027023	Jãa tɩ̃sɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na so ka n tʋ̃nɔ̃ a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ tʋ̃n a wʋ malaka ka wʋ wa ara a n lõboor,
44027024	na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ma, 'Pɔɔl taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, fʋn nyɛn a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa nɩ nɩbir ka wʋ tɔɔr a fʋ 'yɛr. Ka a bala jaa fʋn lɔ̃ɔ chiin Nãaŋmɩn den a ba nyɛvʋr 'yɔ̃ɔ a fʋ nũu pɔ.'
44027025	A lɛ jũu yɩ nyɔɔ nyãa nɩbɛ, n sɔɔn de Nãaŋmɩn ɩka wʋn ɩ naa a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr kʋ ma.
44027026	Tɩchɛ sɩn don dõdol kɔ̃ɔ ju ara."
44027027	A ber pie nɩ anaar daar, a sɛsɛbɛ chɛnɛ na mʋɔrɔ nɩ sɩ be a Adiriya man yal pɔ, a tɩ̃sɔɔ bɩ̃ɩn ka a bala na kaara a gboro tɩɛr man tãa ba gbʋrɔ na gogoro.
44027028	Ba den a bon 'lɔ ban ma mana nɩ a kʋ̃ɔ, man ka a man yulʋ̃fʋ ɩ gbɛɛ kɔbaa dɔɔl lɩjɛr (120). Ban wa chen bɩ̃lãa ba lɛ man kaa ka a yulʋ̃fʋ lɛ ɩ gbɛɛ lɩjaanaar nɩ pie (90).
44027029	Ba joro na dãbɩ̃ɛ ɩka a gboro wʋ taa tɔ̃n sɩ kʋsɩr ɛ, a ba wɛl a nɛbie ala anaar na ma nyɔɔ a gboro lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ a man pɔ tɩ pãa sʋɔrɔ ɩka wɛr wʋ chaar fɔɔ.
44027030	Ka a gboro dẽme bʋɔrɔ sɔr ban na yi a gboro pɔ jo na ba for a gborbile bar ka wʋ suu a man pɔ tɩ maala fɩka a nɛbinyɔɔrsɩ ala lɛ ba foro bara a niem.
44027031	A Pɔɔl pãa 'yɛr kʋ a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a sojasɩ, "Yɩn baa vɛ̃ ka a gboro dẽme banyãna be a gboro pɔ ɛ, sɩ wɛ naa a lɛ nɛ."
44027032	Ka a sojasɩ ŋmaa a miir 'lɔ na nyɔɔ a gborbile taa lɛ ka wʋ lo.
44027033	Lɛ a wɛr na ɩrɛ a wa lalala, Pɔɔl sʋɔr ba jaa na wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩ di a bʋ̃diir bojũu ber pie nɩ anaar nɩ nyã yɩn jɛ̃n baal na yaa di bon jaa ɛ.
44027034	Pʋ̃pãanyã, n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa ɩka yɩ di a bʋ̃diir na yɩ tara kpɛ̃ɔ, a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa jukɔɔlbir kʋ̃ vʋ̃ɔ a wʋ ju pɔ ɛ."
44027035	A anyãna lɛ wʋ 'yɛr baar tɩ na wʋ de a paanʋ̃ɔ amɩne puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan a ba jaa niem, tɩ pãa ŋmaa na wʋ ɔɔrɔ.
44027036	Ka a 'yɔ̃ɔ ba jaa ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɛ ka a ba mɩ̃ɛ di a bʋ̃diir amɩne.
44027037	A sɩn bala na be a gboro pɔ ɩ naa nɩbɛ kɔɔr ayi dɔɔl lɩjaata nɩ pie nɩ ayʋɔb (276).
44027038	Lɛ ban wa di tɩɩ baar, ba wɛl a bʋ̃diir ala na chɛ lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ a man pɔ tɩchɛ ka a gboro ɩ dẽfere.
44027039	Lɛ a wɛr na wa chaar, baa bɔ̃ɔ a jie ban be ɛ, tɩchɛ na ba nyɛ a jie na gɔr ka a bire be be a ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka ala ɩ ba tʋ̃ɔ naa a ba tɩ ara.
44027040	Ba ŋman a mibe ala na nyɔɔr a nɛbinyɔɔrsɩ ala bar, na ba mɩ lɛ for a vuulsɩ ala na ma dɛnɛ a gboro tɩ pãa yɛr a fɔbaa bar a gboro niem ka a sɛsɛbɛ pãa tɔɔrɔ ba chiine a bire pɔ.
44027041	Tɩchɛ ka a gboro tɩ tɔ a bire na duo a jie ɩ̃sʋɔ, ka a gboro niem mʋr wʋ jaa na wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ chen ɛ. Ka a kɔ̃sɛbɛ ŋmiere a gboro pãa wɛlɛ.
44027042	Ka a sojasɩ ɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba kʋ a bala ban pɔɔ ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa dũu yi jo ɛ.
44027043	Tɩchɛ a sojasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ faa a Pɔɔl jũu, waa sɔɔ ɩka ba ɩ a lɛ ɛ. Wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ naa a bala na bɔ̃ɔ a dũufʋ ka ba ɔɔ lo a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ de nie dũu do a gogoro ju.
44027044	Ka a bala na chɛ mɩ nyɔɔr a gboro daar bɩɩ a gboro da'mɛlɛ ala, nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ba ɩ ka ba ɩ̃sʋɔ tɩ jaa do a gogoro ju ka yele ba tara ba ɛ.
44028001	Sɩ jaa na wa do baar, ba 'yɛr ɩka a dõdol yuor din Malta.
44028002	A nɩbɛ bala na be a be maal sɩn vɩla, ba gbɔɔn bũu na ba bʋɔl sɩ a sɩ tɩ uoro, bojũu saa lɛ waara ka ɔɔr kʋrɔ.
44028003	Ka a Pɔɔl mɩ vaar delsɩ wa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bũu pɔ, ka a dʋ̃pãn na be a delsɩ pɔ, a bũu tʋl kpɛ ka wʋ yi dʋ̃ a Pɔɔl nũu mar taalɛ.
44028004	Lɛ a gogoro dẽme bala na wa nyɛ a lɛ a waa na mar a Pɔɔl nũu pɔ jɔ̃jɔlɔ, ka ba 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "A daba nyãna na ɩn nɩkʋrɔ, a man na ba di wʋ gba ɛ, tɩchɛ yeltorsɩ kʋ̃ sɔɔ ka wʋ be be ɛ."
44028005	Tɩchɛ ka a Pɔɔl mɩr a waa 'yɔ̃ɔ a bũu pɔ tɩ yele jaa ba tara wʋ ɛ.
44028006	A nɩbɛ tɩɛr man tãa a nũu na mɔr wʋ naa bɩɩ a wʋ vaa lo kpi. Tɩchɛ ban chɛl lɛ̃ɛɛ wa faa ka a yele jaa ba ɩrɛ ɛ, ba lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ taa, "Ŋmɩn lɛ wʋ ɩ."
44028007	A dõdol 'lɔ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ban bʋɔlɔ Pubilusɩ tara na jie na gbʋr a be a wʋ de sɩ sãan, na wʋ kʋ sɩ bʋ̃diir ber ata.
44028008	A Pubilusɩ sãa bɩɛrɛ na gã, ɩ̃gãn tʋl nɩ masʋmɔ̃ lɛ wʋ nyɩɛrɛ. Pɔɔl kpɛ̃n tɩ nyɛ wʋ, wʋn wa sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn baar wʋ dɔɔl wʋ naa nũu sãa wʋ.
44028009	Lɛ a anyãna na wa ɩ, baalsɩ bala jaa na be a jie 'lɔ mɩ wa naa ka Pɔɔl sãa ba jaa baalsɩ.
44028010	Ba den 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋ sɩ sɔɩ jaa pɔ, a lɛ sɩn wa chɔɔr na yi, ba kʋ sɩn bon jaa sɩn na bʋɔrɔ.
44028011	Sɩ maal a be ŋmɛrsɩ ata tɩ na sɩ lɛ kpɛ a gboro ɩ̃sʋɔ na ara a be a sɩ̃ɛ. A gboro yin Aleksandiriya na wʋ tara ŋmɩn yɩbɛ Kasɩtor nɩ Poluksɩ.
44028012	Sɩ tɩ ara naa Sɩrakusɩ maal ber ata a be.
44028013	Be lɛ a gboro yin sɩ tãn a be a Wuregiyum. Wɛr na wa chaar ka a ɩ a guba jie sɛsɛbɛ furo naa, a ber ayi daar ka sɩ ta a be Puteyoli na sɩ suu a be.
44028014	Be lɛ sɩ pɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo bamɩne ka ba bʋɔl sɩ ka sɩ tɩ maal daa gbul a ba sɛ̃. Lɛ lɛ a ɩ tɩ sɩ pãa wa ta a Worom.
44028015	A Nãaŋmɩn puorbo na be a Worom na wa wõ ɩka sɩ waara naa, ba yin tuor sɩ tɩ ta Apiyusɩ Daa pɔ na ba pɔɔ sɩ a Sãanba Kpɛfʋ Jiir Ata. A lɛ a Pɔɔl na wa nyɛ a nɩbɛ banyãna wʋ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan ka a 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ.
44028016	Lɛ sɩn wa ta a Worom, ba sɔɔ naa ka a Pɔɔl kpɩɛrɛ a wʋ yõ tɩchɛ ka a soja kaara wʋ.
44028017	Pɔɔl na wa maal ber ata, wʋ bʋɔl naa a Juu nɩbɛ nɩdierbe lɔ̃ɔ taa. Lɛ ban wa duo ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "N yɛɛr, n gba na ba maal yele jaa bɔr a sɩ nɩbɛ sɛ̃ ɛ, bɩɩ 'mab a sɩ sãakpãmɩne yel-ɩrsɩ ɛ, tɩ ba nyɔɔ ma naa be a Jerusalɛm na ba kʋ a Worom nɩbɛ.
44028018	Ba chɛ̃pɛ̃n a yele faa na ba ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bar ma bojũu n ba maal yele jaa na sɛɛn kũu ɛ.
44028019	Tɩchɛ ka a Juu nɩbɛ na ba sɔɔ ɛ, ka n faa tɩ sʋɔr sɔr ka ba chiin ma a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa sɛ̃. A ba ɩ n tara na yele kɔ̃ɔ na de dɔɔl a n nɩbɛ ɛ.
44028020	A lɛ jũu lɛ so ka n bʋɔrɔ ɩka n nyɛ yɩ naa 'yɛr yɩ. Bojũu a Isɩral nɩbɛ tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie jũu lɛ ba gbar ma nɩ a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ anyãna."
44028021	Ka ba 'yɛr, "Saa nyɛ gãn jaa yi a Judiya dẽme sɛ̃ ɛ, ka a sɩ yɛɛr bala mɩ na yi a be wa ba 'yɛr a fʋ 'yɛrdɛɛr jaa kʋ sɩ ɛ.
44028022	Tɩchɛ sɩn bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka sɩ bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ fʋn nyɔɔ, bojũu sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka jie jaa nɩbɛ 'laar naa a yele nyãna."
44028023	Ba 'yɔ̃ɔn bɩbir ban lɛ wa a Pɔɔl sɛ̃, a bɩbir na wa vɩɛ ba wan yɔɔ jaa a be wʋn kpɩɛrɛ. An yi a bibio tɩ tãn a jãanʋɔr na wʋ mana a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ kʋrɔ ba, na wʋ de a Mosesɩ nɛɛ nɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na sɛb bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr ka ba sɔɔ a Yesu.
44028024	Bamɩne lɩɛb ba tɩɛr a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr, tɩchɛ ka a bamɩne ba sɔɔ de ɛ.
44028025	Ba chɩrɛ nɩ taa na ba piel yire lɛ a Pɔɔl na wa 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr baaraa na wʋ 'yɛr, "A Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr yelmɩ̃ɛ kʋ a yɩ sãakpãmɩne a lɛ wʋn de a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Isaiya nɛɛ
44028026	'yɛr, 'Chen a nɩbɛ banyãna sɛ̃ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ba, "Yɩn wõn lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ yɩ kʋ̃ wa bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, yɩn fur nɩbir 'yɔ̃ɔ tɩ yɩ kʋ wa nyɛ bon jaa ɛ."
44028027	Bojũu a nɩbɛ banyãna nyãn kpɛ̃mɛ naa, baa wõnõ ɛ, ba ma ũun a ba nɩbie, ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, ban taa nyɛn naa ba nɩbie na ba wõn a ba tobo bɔ̃ɔ a par na ba lɩɛb wa a n sɛ̃ ka n sãa ba.'
44028028	A lɛ jũu, n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn den a wʋ faafʋ 'yɛr tɩ kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ na chɛlɛ naa."
44028030	Pɔɔl yab a yir 'lɔ pɔ wʋn kpɩɛrɛ yuom ayi, tɩ ma de nɩrɛ jaa na ma wa a wʋ sɛ̃.
44028031	Yele jaa ba ŋmaa wʋ sɔr ɛ, ka wʋ 'lara na wʋ mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ 'yɛr na wʋ wile ba nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr.
45001001	Maa Pɔɔl na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto gbãgbaa, Nãaŋmɩn na kaa ir bʋɔl ka n ɩ a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nãa naa ɩ a wʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ, lɛ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ a yɩn na be a Worom.
45001002	A 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã wʋn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr nɛɛ a kõr jaa tu a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ sɛ̃ ka ba sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ,
45001003	na ɩ a wʋ Bie 'yɛr, ban dɔɔ ka wʋ ɩ a Nãa David bal nɩrɛ.
45001004	A tu naa a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pɔ wiil kpɛ̃ɔ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn Bie lɛ, na wʋ ir yi a kũn pɔ ɩ vʋr, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ Soro.
45001005	A tun a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩ a wʋ yuor jũu, sɩ nyɛn wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ na sɩn bʋɔl nɩrɛ jaa, ka ba wa wõnõ a wʋ toor nɩ sɔɔfʋ.
45001006	Yɩn mɩ pʋɔn a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl ka yɩ ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sofʋ.
45001007	N sɛɛrɛ na kʋrɔ a yɩn bala jaa na be a Worom a Nãaŋmɩn na nʋ̃, na wʋ bʋɔl yɩ a yɩ ɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jie a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
45001008	N den nie puor a maa Nãaŋmɩn yãan a yɩ jaa jũu tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, bojũu a yɩ sɔɔfʋ ŋmen yaar a wɛr wʋ jaa.
45001009	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã ɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ nɩ a n nyãa wʋ jaa, naa mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã na ɩ a wʋ Bie 'yɛr, di man dãasɩɛ lɛ ɩn ma tɩɛrɛ a yɩ yele.
45001010	N ma sʋɔrɔ naa Nãaŋmɩn ba gala ɛ, naa sʋɔrɔ ɩka a wʋ bɔfʋ a ɩ, ka wʋ yuo sɔr a pʋ̃pãanyã kʋ ma ka n wa a yɩ sɛ̃.
45001011	N bʋɔrɔ naa yɩ nyɛfʋ naa na tʋ̃ɔ wiil yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋfʋ amɩne ka a 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ.
45001012	Lɛ lɛ, a yɩn nɩ maa na pãa nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ̃mɛ a sɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ.
45001013	N yɛɛr, n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ ɩn mʋɔrɔ sɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ jaa, ɩka n wa a yɩ sɛ̃ tɩchɛ ka a sɔr pɔɔ wa tãn dɩna. Ɩn taa nyɛn a yɩ bamɩne a ba puoraa nɩtãa lɛ ɩn nyɛ a yɩ bamɩne na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, tɩ puoro.
45001014	N din a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala mɩ na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, nɩ a yɛ̃ dẽme nɩ a jɔlɔ sãn.
45001015	Ala lɛ so ka n mʋɔrɔ ɩka n mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ a yɩn mɩ na be a Worom.
45001016	Vɩ̃ ba kʋrɔ ma nɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna 'yɛrfʋ ɛ, bojũu a ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ wʋn de faara nɩ nɩrɛ jaa na sɔɔ, a Juu nɩbɛ lɛ de nie, ka bala mɩ na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, mɩ tu.
45001017	Bojũu a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã na wiil nɩrɛ lɛ wʋn na tor Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, torfʋ 'lɔ na yi sɔɔfʋ pɔ, yi a pielfʋ tɩ tãn a baaraa nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara sɔɔfʋ, tor naa, wʋn tara na nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ."
45001018	Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃n ka a wʋ suur yele yi a saaju gã chãa pɔ, ɩka wʋ nyɛn suur 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na ba puoro ɛ, nɩ putudẽme bala na pɔɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a ba putuyele.
