45001019	An ɩ a ala ban na de bɔ̃ɔn a Nãaŋmɩn gãn chãa pɔ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ ir wiil ba.
45001020	Bojũu, an yi a lɛ daar jaa a Nãaŋmɩn na mɛ a wɛr, nɩbɛ na tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, ka wʋ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bonsɩ ala wʋn maal, a lɛ jũu, tu yifʋ jie ba lɛ be be go ɛ.
45001021	Bojũu, ban sɔɔ bɔ̃ɔn a Nãaŋmɩn a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃, tɩ baa kʋ wʋ tɩɩr ɛ, bɩɩ dãna wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a ba tɩɛrsɩ ɩn burbur, ka a ba jɔl nyãn ala pãa lii.
45001022	Ban sɔɔ 'yɛr ɩka yɛ̃ bɔ̃ɔnbɔ lɛ ba ɩ, ba ɩn jɔlɔ,
45001023	an ɩ ba lɩɛb a tɩɩr 'lɔ ban taa kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ba kpire ɛ, na ba kʋ a bʋtɩbɛ ala ban pɛ̃n, ka a kaara a nɩbɛ kaar na kpire, nɩ lubil, nɩ dʋ̃n, nɩ dʋ̃gbɛɛ anaar jaa bʋrɔ.
45001024	Ala lɛ so ka Nãaŋmɩn ir nũu tɩchɛ ba bar be a ba vɔldɛɛr pɔ, ka ba bʋ̃nɔ̃ gãna nɩ taa, sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa nɩ a ba ɩ̃gãma.
45001025	Ba den a Nãaŋmɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ tɛɛn jire, na ba puoro tɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a bonsɩ ala a Nãaŋmɩn na maal, tɩ bar a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a ma maala 'lɔ a pɛɛfʋ na sɛɛn bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
45001026	A anyãna jũu, Nãaŋmɩn de ban bar be a vɩ̃ vɔlaa pɔ. Ka a ba pɔbɔ gba ma lɩɛb gãna nɩ a ba pɔɔ taa ba.
45001027	A lɛ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ a dɔɔr mɩ bar a pɔbɔ bɔfʋ, ka a vɔlaa vɛ̃ ka ba lɩɛb bʋɔrɔ a ba taa dɔɔr. Dɔɔr na lɩɛb tʋ̃nɔ̃ a vɩ̃ tʋ̃mɔ̃ nyãna nɩ a ba taa dɔɔr ba nyɛn a ba tʋ̃dɛɛr toor tɔɔfʋ.
45001028	Baa nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔ̃ɔfʋ a wʋ sɛɛn ba ɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn bar ba a be a ba tɩɛr sɔ̃ɔnaa pɔ, ka ba maala a ala na ba sɛɛn maalfʋ ɛ.
45001029	Ba sɛɛn naa putuo jaa bʋrɔ, bier ɩfʋ, bɔgar dẽme, nɩ bier maalfʋ. Nyuur sɛɛn ba naa, na ba ɩ nɩkʋrbɔ, bʋɔrɔ jɛɛr, na ba bɛlɛ taa, na ba tɩɛrɛ taa sɔ̃ɔfʋ. Ba ɩn gagarsɩ,
45001030	sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ taa yoe, 'laar Nãaŋmɩn, kpɛrɛ taa, mɩ̃ɛ 'mɔɔfʋ nɩ yobɔyele. Ba bɔ̃ɔn sɔɩ ban ma tu maal bier, baa turo a nɩbɛ bala na dɔɔ ba nɛɛ ɛ.
45001031	Baa tara tɩɛr ɛ, baa tara yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, baa tara nʋ̃fʋ ɛ, baa kaara nɩrɛ nɩbaal ɛ.
45001032	Ban sɔɔ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn toraa nyãna binfʋ, ɩka a nɩbɛ bala na maala a anyãna sɛɛn nɩ kũu, bala mɩ̃ɛ tɛɛ ba lɛ maala a anyãna ɛ, tɩchɛ ba ma sɔɔ naa a bala na tʋ̃nɔ̃ a anyãna.
45002001	Yɩn a lɛ jũu, yaa mɩ tara tu yifʋ jie ɛ, a yɩn bala na ma tɔɔrɔ a bamɩne 'yɛr. Yele jaa pɔ fʋn tɔɔr a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ 'yɛr fʋ mɩ 'yɔ̃ɔn fʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr, bojũu fʋ mɩ ɩn a yele 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ na ɩ, a fʋ tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr.
45002002	Pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na tɔɔr naa a bala na ɩrɛ a yelsɩ anyãna 'yɛr tun yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔr pɔ.
45002003	A lɛ a fʋ̃ʋ nɩsaal mɩ na tɔɔrɔ nɩbɛ 'yɛr, tɩ na fʋ mɩ maal a yele ala nɩ a ju, fʋ tɩɛr ɩka fʋn pɔl yi a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ pɔ ɔ?
45002004	Bɩɩ yɩ nyɛ naa Nãaŋmɩn yɛ̃ bɔ̃ɔn yɔɔ jũu, nɩ a wʋ maalvɩla, nɩ a wʋ kãnyir, na yaa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn maalvɩla wile yɩn tɩɛr lɩɛb fʋ sɔr ɛ?
45002005	Tɩchɛ a yɩ nyãkpɩ̃ɛn nɩ yɩn ba lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr jũu, yɩ guoro naa a Nãaŋmɩn sutuo bine kʋrɔ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ guro nɩ a wʋ suur bɩbir 'lɔ wʋn na tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr nɩ torfʋ.
45002006	Nãaŋmɩn "na yab nɩrɛ jaa lɛ wʋn tũ jɩ̃."
45002007	Bala na mar ara na ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ vɩla bʋɔrɔ tɩɩr, nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, nɩ a ala na ba pʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ, wʋn kʋ ban nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
45002008	Tɩchɛ bala na bʋɔrɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ bɔb, na ba tɔr a yelmɩ̃ɛ tɩ turo dɛɛr, Nãaŋmɩn suur nɩ a wʋ kpãafʋ gãn kʋ ba.
45002009	Wõm nɩ tuo difʋ na ben be kʋ nɩsaal jaa na ɩrɛ yelbier. An piel naa a Juu nɩbɛ sɛ̃, tɩ mɩ lʋ̃ɔ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ.
45002010	Tɩchɛ tɩɩr nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na ben be kʋ nɩrɛ jaa na maala vɩla, a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ.
45002011	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn ba tara kaa gar taa ɛ.
45002012	Bala jaa na ba bɔ̃ɔ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ tɩ tʋ̃ dɛɛr, mɩn wɛ naa ban ba bɔ̃ɔ a nɛɛ jũu, ka bala jaa mɩn bɔ̃ɔ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ tɩ tʋ̃ a dɛɛr Nãaŋmɩn na den a nɛɛ nyã tɔɔr a ba 'yɛr.
45002013	Bojũu a ba ɩ a bala na wõnõ a nɛɛ lɛ tor a Nãaŋmɩn niem ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala na turo a lɛ a nɛɛ na 'yɛr bala lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛr ɩka ba tor naa.
45002014	Sɩrɛ jaa a bala jaa na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, na baa tara a Mosesɩ nɛbinãa ɛ, ba gba ma ɩ naa a yelsɩ a nɛɛ na 'yɛr, bojũu bala mɩ̃ɛ ɩn a nɛɛ ban sɔɔ ba tara a nɛɛ ɛ.
45002015	Ba wiil ɩka a lɛ a nɛɛ na bʋɔrɔ sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ be a ba nyãa pɔ, ka a ba tɩɛr mɩ di dãasɩɛ ma gɔ̃nɔ̃ ba bɩɩ 'yɛrɛ pʋɔrɔ ba.
45002016	A anyãna na ɩ naa a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn na tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ na wʋ tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa yelsɔɔlsɩ nɩtãa lɛ ɩn 'yɛrɛ a n 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ.
45002017	Pʋ̃pãanyã a fʋ̃ʋ, ala ɩ fʋ bʋɔlɔ na a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ Juu nɩrɛ, na fʋ dɩɛl a Mosesɩ nɛɛ na fʋ jɩrɛ lɛ fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn na tara nɛbʋ̃'yen,
45002018	ala ɩ fʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa a wʋ bɔfʋ na fʋ bɔ̃ɔ a 'lɔ na gar a jaa bojũu a nɛɛ lɛ wiil fʋ,
45002019	ala ɩ fʋ chɛn nyãa ɩka jɔ̃tɔɔrɔ lɛ fʋ ɩ, na fʋ ɩ chãa chaara a bala na be a libe pɔ,
45002020	na fʋ wile a jɔlɔ, na fʋ wile a bibiir, bojũu a Mosesɩ nɛɛ pɔ lɛ fʋ nyɛ a bɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ.
45002021	Fʋ̃ʋ nyã na wile a fʋ taaba, faa wiil a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ? Fʋ̃ʋ nyã na ma 'yɛrɛ ɩka jufʋ ba ɩ ɛ, fʋ ma ju naa ɔ?
45002022	Fʋ̃ʋ na ma 'yɛrɛ ɩka nɩbɛ ba ta sɛ̃nɛ ɛ, fʋ ma sɛ̃n bɩɩ? Fʋ̃ʋ nyã na kpɛrɛ a tɩbɛ tɩ fʋ ma juro naa a tɩbɛ der bonsɩ bɩɩ?
45002023	Fʋ̃ʋ nyã na jɩrɛ nɩ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ nyã, fʋ ma 'yɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn vɩ̃ fʋn sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nɛɛ ɔ?
45002024	Nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "A yɩ jũu lɛ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a n yuor."
45002025	Yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ tara na tɔ̃nɔ̃ ala ɩ fʋ turo naa lɛ a nɛɛ na 'yɛr, tɩchɛ ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ baa turo a nɛɛ ɛ, fʋn kaara fɩka faa ŋmaa yʋɔr ɛ.
45002026	Ala ɩ a bala na ba ŋmaa a yʋɔr ɛ, turo na lɛ a nɛɛ na bin, ba kʋ̃ kaara fɩka yɔŋmarba lɛ ba ɩ ɛ?
45002027	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba ŋmaa a yʋɔr a ɩ̃gãn pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ na wʋ turo a nɛɛ jaa nɛ nɛ nɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩn 'yɛr, a yɩn bala gba na tara a nɛbinsɩ gãn na fʋ ŋmaa a yʋɔr tɩ faa turo a nɛbinsɩ ɛ.
45002028	Nɩrɛ na ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ ba ɩ a ɩ̃gãn nyã yele tɛɛ lɛ ɛ, bɩɩ a yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ na ɩ a ɩ̃gãn yele ɛ.
45002029	Kai, wʋ ɩn a Juu nɩrɛ na be a pʋɔm, ka a wʋ yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na ŋmaa a wʋ nyãa yʋɔr a ba yi a nɛbinsɩ gãn pɔ ɛ. A nɩrɛ nyãna pɛɛfʋ ba yire nɩbɛ sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yin Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
45003001	Bo tɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a Juu nɩrɛ tara, bɩɩ bo tɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ be be a yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ pɔ?
45003002	Sɔr jaa pɔ, ala na de nie lɛ ɩka bala lɛ Nãaŋmɩn de nie kʋ a wʋ 'yɛrbie.
45003003	Bo lɛ na ɩ ala ɩ bamɩne ba tara sɔɔfʋ ɛ? A ba ba sɔɔfʋ na tʋ̃ɔn sɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ bar bɩɩ?
45003004	Kai, sɔr ba be be ɛ! Vɛ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, tɩchɛ ka a nɩrɛ jaa ɩ jir ŋmara. Nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Lɛ lɛ na wiil ɩka fʋ tor naa a fʋ 'yɛrbie pɔ, na fʋ tʋ̃ɔ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie."
45003005	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a sɩ ba torfʋ vɛ̃n ka Nãaŋmɩn torfʋ gã chãa pɔ, sɩ lɛ 'yɛr bo? Sɩ 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn ba tor ɛ, wʋn vɛ̃ ka a wʋ sutuo dire sɩ ɔ? Nɩsaal nɛchɩrɛ lɛ a nyãna.
45003006	Sɩrɛ jaa ba lɛ ɛ. Ala ɩ lɛ lɛ, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ tɔɔr a wɛr nɩbɛ 'yɛr?
45003007	Nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na chɩrɛ na, "Ka ala ɩ a n ba torfʋ wiil naa ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ ka a wʋ tɩɩr pʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ, bãa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ma 'yɛr ɩka yelbe-ɩrɛ lɛ n ɩ?"
45003008	Bo lɛ so ka sɩ kʋ̃ 'yɛr nɩtãa lɛ a yosɔ̃ɔnbɔ na 'yɛr ka a bamɩne mɩ 'yɛrɛ ɩka sɩ 'yɛr ɩka, "Yɩ ɩ a sɩ maala dɛɛr tɩ ka a lɩɛrɛ vɩla?" A ba sɔ̃ɔfʋ sɛɛn ba naa.
45003009	Bãa lɛ sɩn pãa de baar? Sɩn lɛ sa ba bɩɩ? Kai, sɔr ba be be ɛ. Sɩ den nie 'yɛr ɩka a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ba jaa nyɛntaa na ba be a yelbier pɔ.
45003010	Nɩtãa lɛ ban sɛb a ba yele 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Nɩtoraa jaa ba be be ɛ, nɩbʋ̃'yen gba ba be be ɛ.
45003011	Nɩbʋ̃'yen jaa ba be be bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ 'yɛr par ɛ, nɩbʋ̃'yen jaa ba yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ.
45003012	Ba jaa lɩɛb puor, ka ba jaa lɩɛb ɩ nɩsɔ̃ɔnsɩ. Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba maala vɩla ɛ, nɩbʋ̃'yen gba ba be be ɛ."
45003013	"A ba kɔkɔbɔɔr yuon fɩka yar, ka a ba jãlbie bɔ̃ɔ bɛlfʋ." "Dʋ̃pãn lɔɔ jɛlaa a ba nɛgãma."
45003014	"Pɔ'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ 'yɛr bitor lɛ ma yire a ba nɛɛr pɔ."
45003015	"A ba gbɛɛ ma pɔɔrɔ naa jɩ̃ɩ kpaarfʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
45003016	Sɔr jaa ban de, sɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ dɔɔyɛ lɛ ma ɩ a jɩ̃nɛ.
45003017	Baa bɔ̃ɔ nyã'maar sɔr ɛ."
45003018	"A ba nɩbie ba joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ."
45003019	Pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka lɛ jaa a Mosesɩ nɛɛ na 'yɛr, wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a bala na be a nɛɛ pɔ ɩka, a kpal nɩrɛ jaa nɛɛ, ka a wɛr nɩbɛ ba jaa wa man a ba nɛɛ 'yɛr kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn.
45003020	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ ɩ nɩtor a Nãaŋmɩn niem wʋn turo a nɛɛ jũu ɛ, an ɩ a tun a nɛɛ nyã pɔ, ka sɩ bɔ̃ɔ bier.
45003021	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, a chaar naa ɩka a torfʋ na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, ba yi a Mosesɩ nɛɛ pɔ ɛ, ala lɛ a nɛɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ di dãasɩɛ.
45003022	A torfʋ nyã na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, ɩn a sɔɔfʋ na tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, kʋ a bala jaa na sɔɔ de. Tɛɛ taa jaa ba be be ɛ.
45003023	Bojũu nɩrɛ jaa maal dɛɛr na baa ta a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr ɛ.
45003024	A Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu, wʋ vɛ̃n ka sɩ tor na wʋ 'yɛrfaa sɩ pɔrɔ tu a faafʋ 'lɔ na yi a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃.
45003025	Nãaŋmɩn de wʋn a wʋ ɩ a bɔɔrlo bon, a wʋn de a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ pɛɛn nɩrɛ jaa tu a sɔɔfʋ jũu. Nãaŋmɩn maal a anyã na wʋ wiil a wʋ torfʋ, bojũu a wʋ kãnyir vɛ̃ naa ka wʋ bar a ba yeldɛbɛ ala ban dɔ̃ɔ maal gefʋ.
45003026	Wʋ maal naa lɛ na wiil a wʋ torfʋ a pʋ̃pãanyã, na wʋ ma vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa na sɔɔ de a Yesu yele, tor.
45003027	Nyɩnɛ lɛ a yobɔyele lɛ be? A ba pʋɔ be ɛ. Yelbuor jũu? A Mosesɩ nɛɛ ban turo jũu bɩɩ? Kai, sɔɔfʋ jũu lɛ.
45003028	Ala lɛ so ka sɩn chɛnɛ sɔɔ ɩka nɩrɛ yele ma tor naa wʋn tara sɔɔfʋ a ba ɩ wʋn turo a nɛbinãa jũu ɛ.
45003029	Nãaŋmɩn ɩn a Juu nɩbɛ tɛɛ Nãaŋmɩn bɩɩ? Waa ɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ mɩ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ? Ɔ̃ɔ, wʋ ɩn a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ mɩ tʋɔr.
45003030	An ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ be be, 'lɔ lɛ na vɛ̃ ka a yɔŋmarba yele tor sɔɔfʋ jũu, na wʋ mɩ vɛ̃ ka a bala na ba ŋmaa a yʋɔr ɛ, yele mɩ tor a sɔɔfʋ jũu.
45003031	Sɩ pãa den a sɔɔfʋ nyã sɔ̃ɔn a nɛbinãa bar bɩɩ? Kai, sɔr ba be be ɛ. Sɩn lɛ pãa bɔ̃ɔ turo wʋ.
45004001	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ sɩn pãa 'yɛr a sɩ sãakpã Abraham 'yɛr, a yele nyãna pɔ?
45004002	Ala ɩ sɩrɛ jaa Abraham yele dɔ̃ɔ tor a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ jũu, wʋn taa tara na yele kɔ̃ɔ bʋɔrɔ nɩ yuor, tɩchɛ a kʋ̃ naa ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn niem lɛ ɛ.
45004003	Bo lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn 'yɛr? Wʋ 'yɛr ɩka, "Abraham sɔɔn de Nãaŋmɩn ka a lɛ vɛ̃ ka wʋ ɩ nɩtor."
45004004	Pʋ̃pãanyã nɩrɛ wa tʋ̃tʋ̃mɔ̃, a wʋ sãyar ba ɩ kʋfʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ sãyar lɛ.
45004005	Ala lɛ so nɩrɛ 'lɔ an ba ɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋn sɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ na ma vɛ̃ ka a putudẽme yele tor, a wʋ sɔɔfʋ lɛ ma vɛ̃ ka wʋ ɩ a nɩtor.
45004006	A Nãa David mɩ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a 'yɛr bir nyãna nɩ wʋ ju, na wʋ 'yɛr ɩka, bɔɔsʋ̃n sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ a wʋ ɩ nɩtor ka tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba pʋɔ ɛ.
45004007	"Bɔɔsʋ̃n dẽme lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ a ba bɔrfʋsɩ kʋ ba, ka a ba yelbebe ala pɔɔ.
45004008	Bɔɔsʋ̃n lɛ a 'lɔ a sɩ Soro na ba lɛ sɔrɔ a wʋ yelbier dɔɔlɔ wʋ ɛ."
45004009	A bɔɔsʋ̃n nyãna ɩn a yɔŋmarba tɛɛ bon bɩɩ, a mɩ ɩn a bala na ba ŋmaa a yʋɔr ɛ, bon? Sɩ 'yɛr ɩka Abraham sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃n ka wʋ ɩ nɩtor.
45004010	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ anyãna dɔ̃ɔ ɩ kʋ wʋ? Wʋn ŋmaa a yʋɔr baar lɛ bɩɩ wʋn ba ŋmaa sɛrɛ lɛ? A ba ɩ wʋn ŋmaa baar ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ ba ŋmaa sɛrɛ lɛ.
45004011	Nãaŋmɩn wa bɩɛr man wʋ a yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ yele, ka a ɩ jɩ̃nɛ ɩka a wʋ yele tor naa a wʋ sɔɔfʋ jũu wʋn dɔ̃ɔ ba ŋmaa a yʋɔr sɛrɛ ɛ. Lɛ lɛ wʋ pãa ɩ a bala jaa na sɔɔ de sãa, tɩchɛ na baa ŋmaa a ba yɔɩ ɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃ a ba ɩ nɩtorsɩ.
45004012	Wʋ mɩ ɩ naa bala jaa na ŋma a yɔɩ sãa. A ba ɩ yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ tɛɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ ban tara a sɔɔfʋ na ba turo nɩ a lɛ a sɩ sãa Abraham na dɔ̃ɔ turo tɩ wa ŋmaa a yʋɔr.
45004013	A ba ɩ a nɛbinãa jũu lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a Abraham nɩ a wʋ yɔn ɩka bala lɛ na so a wɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋn ɩ nɩtor a wʋ sɔɔfʋ jũu lɛ.
45004014	Ala ɩ a bala na turo a nɛbinãa lɛ so a wɛr ɛ, sɔɔfʋ ba lɛ tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ wʋn tɩr mɩ ɩ pɔrɔ.
45004015	Bojũu a nɛbinãa waara nɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn suur. A jie 'lɔ mɩ a nɛbinãa na ba be ɛ, a nɛɛ bɔrfʋsɩ mɩ ba be be ɛ.
45004016	A lɛ jũu, a nɛtɩraa wa naa a sɔɔfʋ jũu, ka a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ na sʋ̃ʋ a Abraham yɔn ba jaa, a ba ɩ a bala na turo a nɛɛ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala na tara a Abraham sɔɔfʋ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a sɩ jaa sãa.
45004017	Nɩtãa an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "N maal fʋ naa a fʋ ɩ a paal yɔɔ sãa." 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ a sɩ sãa a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, a 'lɔ wʋn sɔɔ de, a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ma vɛ̃ ka kũn ɩ vʋɛ, na wʋ ma bʋɔl bonsɩ ala na ba dɔ̃ɔ be be ɛ, ka a be be.
45004018	Tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie ba lɛ be be ɛ, tɩ Abraham tara tɩɛrtɔ jie, na wʋ sɔɔ de ka a lɛ vɛ̃ ka wʋ ɩ a paal yɔɔ sãa, nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Lɛ lɛ a fʋ yɔn na wa be."
45004019	Waa bal a wʋ sɔɔfʋ pɔ ɛ, wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nyɛn bɔ̃ɔn a wʋ ɩ̃gãn na kor jʋɔl, bojũu yuom kɔbaa lɛ wʋ nyɛ ka a Saara mɩ ab.
45004020	Tɩchɛ Abraham ba tara baal a wʋ sɔɔfʋ pɔ, nɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ nyɛn kpɛ̃ɔ a wʋ sɔɔfʋ pɔ, na wʋ de tɩɩr kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn.
45004021	Wʋ sɔɔn de nuur ayi ɩka Nãaŋmɩn tara na kpɛ̃ɔ na maal a lɛ wʋn tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ.
45004022	A anyãna lɛ so ka a Nãaŋmɩn, vɛ̃ a wʋ ɩ nɩtor.
45004023	A 'yɛrbir na 'yɛr ɩka, Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃n a wʋ ɩ nɩtor, a ba sɛb a 'lɔ tɛɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ,
45004024	tɩchɛ a mɩ ɩn a sɩ bon, Nãaŋmɩn mɩ na vɛ̃n a sɩ yele ka a tor, sɩn bala jaa na sɔɔ ɩka, 'lɔ lɛ sɩ̃ɩ a Yesu na ɩ a sɩ Soro a kũu pɔ.
45004025	A sɩ yelbebe jũu lɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ kʋn wʋ, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a kũu pɔ a wʋ ɩ vʋr, na wʋ vɛ̃ ka sɩ tor.
45005001	Wʋn ben vɛ̃ a sɩ tor a sɩ sɔɔfʋ jũu, sɩ tara na nyã'maar Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ tu a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
45005002	A wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ sɩ tu nyɛ sɔr a sɩ sɔɔfʋ jũu kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ nyã pɔ sɩn ben ara a pʋ̃pãanyã, na sɩ chɩlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr tɩɛrtɔ nyã jũu.
45005003	A ba ɩ lɛ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩ mɩ chɩlɛ na a sɩ dɔɔyɛ pɔ, bojũu sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a dɔɔyɛ lɛ na waan kãnyir,
45005004	ka a kãnyir wiil a lɛ fʋn be, ka a lɛ fʋn be mɩ waan tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie.
45005005	Ka a tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie kʋ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ vɩ̃ ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn kpaar naa a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ nyãn pɔ, tu a wʋ Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn de kʋ sɩ.
45005006	Yaa nyɛ, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ na sɛɛ lɛ, sɩn sɔɔ chɛnɛ ba tara kpɛ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ Kɩrɩsɩto kpin kʋ a bala na ba puoro ɛ.
45005007	An kpɛ̃mɛ naa ɩka nɩrɛ na sɔɔn kpi kʋ nɩrɛ yele na tor, amɩne nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na tʋ̃ɔn sɔɔ kpi kʋ nɩrɛ na ɩ nɩsʋ̃.
45005008	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn wiil a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nʋ̃fʋ a nɩtɔ̃ kʋ sɩ, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn chɛnɛ ɩ yelbe-ɩrbɛ, Kɩrɩsɩto kpin kʋ sɩ.
45005009	An ben ɩka pʋ̃pãanyã wʋ ben vɛ̃ a sɩ tor a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ jũu, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an pãa kaara wʋn faa sɩ yin a Nãaŋmɩn suur pɔ.
45005010	Bojũu ala ɩ a lɛ sɩn dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃dẽme, ka a wʋ Bie kũu wa 'maal wʋ kʋ sɩ, a lɛ wʋn ben 'maal sɩ, wʋn faa sɩ naa tu a wʋ nyɛvʋr pɔ.
45005011	A ba ɩ anyã tɛɛ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩ chɩlɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ tu a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, tu a 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩn ben nyɛ a 'maalfʋ a pʋ̃pãanyã.
45005012	Nɩtɔ̃ jũu lɛ a yelbier kpɛ a wɛr pɔ tu nɩbʋ̃'yen 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a kũu mɩ tu a yelbier 'yɔ̃ɔ mɩ wa, sɔr nyã lɛ a kũu mɩ tu pɔɔ nɩrɛ jaa, bojũu ba jaa maal yelbier.
45005013	Sɛrɛ tɩchɛ ka a Mosesɩ wa bin a nɛɛ, yelbier den nie be ka a wɛr pɔ, tɩchɛ lɛ a nɛbinãa na ba dɔ̃ɔ be be ɛ, ba maa de yelbier maal bon ɛ.
45005014	Tɩchɛ kũu din nãa yi a Adama sɔ̃ɔ tɩ tãn a Mosesɩ sɔ̃ɔ, na wʋ gba mɩ tʋ̃ɔ a bala na ba maal a yelbier sɔ̃ɔ a nɛɛ a Adama kaar ɛ, Adama lɛ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a 'lɔ na wa wa gãagiel.
45005015	Tɩchɛ a kʋfʋ ba kaara a bɔrfʋ kaar ɛ, bojũu ala ɩ nɩyɔɔ kpi naa nɩbʋ̃'yen bɔrfʋ jũu, Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ a wʋ kʋfʋ ala na wa tu a nɩbʋ̃'yen Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu, na yaar kʋ nɩyɔɔ gar a lɛ.
45005016	A Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ gba ba nyɛtãan a nɩbʋ̃'yen yelbier 'lɔ ɛ. 'Yɛr tɔɔrfʋ tun a yelbe bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ na wʋ waan sɔ̃ɔfʋ, tɩchɛ a kʋfʋ mɩ tun a bɔrfʋsɩ yɔɔ pɔ, naa waan torfʋ.
45005017	Bojũu ala ɩ a nɩbʋ̃'yen bɔrfʋ jũu kũu din nãa tu a nɩbʋ̃'yen 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a bala na nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ a kʋfʋ 'lɔ na ɩ a torfʋ, na din nãa a ba nyɛvʋr pɔ tu a nɩbʋ̃'yen Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
45005018	An ɩ nɩbʋ̃'yen bɔrfʋ jũu lɛ waan sɔ̃ɔfʋ wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɩbɛ ba jaa, lɛ lɛ so nɩbʋ̃'yen mɩ na maal ka a tor, mɩ lɛ vɛ̃ ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa tor na ba nyɛ nyɛvʋr.
45005019	Nɩtãa lɛ a bawõno bʋ̃'yen na vɛ̃ ka a nɩyɔɔ ɩ yelbe-ɩrbɛ, lɛ mɩ lɛ a tu nɩbʋ̃'yen na tu Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ mɩ vɛ̃, ka a nɩyɔɔ mɩ ɩ nɩtorsɩ.
45005020	A nɛɛ pʋɔn 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a bɔrfʋsɩ mɩ waa. Tɩchɛ jie 'lɔ a yelbier na pʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ, Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ ma pʋɔn 'yɔ̃ɔ gar a lɛ.
45005021	Nɩtãa lɛ a yelbier na di nãa a kũu pɔ, lɛ mɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ na di a nãa tu a yeltorsɩ pɔ, na wʋ waan nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ.
45006001	Sɩ pãa 'yɛr ɩka bo? Sɩ chɛnɛ ɩrɛ a yelbier tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ pʋɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃?
45006002	Kai, sɔr ba be be ɛ! Sɩ kpin kʋ yelbier, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a ɩ a sɩn lɛ chɛnɛ be a pɔ?
45006003	Bɩɩ yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a sɩn bala jaa na so a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, wʋ pɔl sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ, a sɩ lɔ̃ɔ kpin wʋ nɩ a wʋ kũu pɔ ɛ?
45006004	A lɛ jũu, ba ũu sɩ naa a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ, a kũu kaar, ka a lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na dɔ̃ɔ ir a kũu pɔ, tu a Sãa tɩɩr pɔ, ka sɩ mɩ na be be tara nyɛvʋr paalaa.
45006005	Ala ɩ sɩn nɩ 'lɔ 'mantaa a wʋ kũu pɔ, sɩn nɩ 'lɔ na 'mantaa ir a kũu pɔ.
45006006	Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a sɩ ɩ̃gãn koraa pʋɔ naa a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, a ba kpan wʋ a be a daa ju, ka a yelbier ɩ̃gãn ba lɛ tara kpɛ̃ɔ a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, saa lɛ ɩ a yelbier gbãgbaar ɛ.
45006007	Bojũu nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na kpi, wʋ yin yelbier pɔ.
45006008	Ala ɩ sɩn nɩ Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ 'mataa kpi, sɩ sɔɔ naa ɩka sɩn nɩ 'lɔ lɛ na 'mataa be be tara a nyɛvʋr.
45006009	Bojũu sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a Kɩrɩsɩto na ir a kũu pɔ, wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ kpi go ɛ, kũu ba lɛ tʋ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ.
45006010	A kũu wʋn kpi, wʋ kpin kʋ yelbier gbɛbʋ̃'yen kʋ nɩrɛ jaa, tɩchɛ a wʋ nyɛvʋr pɔ wʋn be, wʋ ben be kʋ Nãaŋmɩn.
45006011	A lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ ɩka, yɩ kaa a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɩka, yɩ kpin kʋ yelbier, tɩ be be kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jũu.
45006012	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta sɔɔ ka yelbier lɛ di nãa a yɩ ɩ̃gãn nyãn na kpi ka yɩ turo a wʋ dɛɛr bɔfʋ ɛ.
45006013	Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa diere a yɩ ɩ̃gãn jie ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋrɔ yelbier maalfʋ ɛ, ka a ɩ putuyele tʋ̃tʋ̃bomo ɛ. Tɩchɛ yɩ sɔɔ de a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn, nɩtãa nɩbɛ na yi kũu pɔ tara nyɛvʋr, na yɩ sɔɔ de a yɩ ɩ̃gãn jiir kʋ wʋ, ka a ɩ yeltorsɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃bomo.
45006014	Bojũu, yelbier ba lɛ ɩ a yɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɛ, bojũu yaa chɛnɛ be a Mosesɩ nɛbinãa pĩlem ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ben a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ pĩlem.
45006015	Ka bo go? Sɩ chɛnɛ ɩrɛ a yelbier bojũu sɩn ba lɛ chɛnɛ be a nɛɛ pĩlem ɔ, tɩ be a wɩ̃ɛfʋ pĩlem bɩɩ? Kai, sɔr ba be be ɛ!
45006016	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka ala ɩ fʋ wa den fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ nɩrɛ na fʋ turo a wʋ nɛɛ gbãgbaa kaar, fʋ ɩn gbãgbaa kʋ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ nɛɛ fʋn turo, ka yelbier gbãgbaa lɛ fʋ ɩ a 'lɔ na chiine a kũu pɔ, bɩɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ tufʋ 'lɔ mɩ na chiine nɩ fʋ a yeltorsɩ jie.
45006017	Tɩchɛ n puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, yɩn dɔ̃ɔ gba ɩ a yelbier gbãgbaar, tɩ yɩ wa sɔɔn naa a yɩ nyãa wʋ jaa na yɩ de a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wiilfʋ nyã pɔ.
45006018	Nãaŋmɩn faa yɩn yin a yelbier pɔ a yɩ so yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, na yɩ lɩɛb yeltorsɩ gbãgbaar.
45006019	Nɩsaal 'yɛr lɛ n de man a yɩ ɩ̃gãma yɩn ba tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ nyɔɔrɔ jũu. Nɩtãa lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ ma de a yɩ ɩ̃gãn jiir ka a ɩ gbãgbaar kʋ a ala na ba vɩɛl ɛ, naa ma pʋɔrɔ putuyele 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃, pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ, yɩ de a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ka a ɩ yeltorsɩ nɩ chɛchɛ ɩfʋ gbãgbaar.
45006020	Yɩn dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a yelbier gbãgbaar, a yeltorsɩ ba so yɩ ɛ.
45006021	Tɔ̃nɔ̃ buor lɛ yɩ nyɛ yin a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a yelsɩ ala na ben ɩ vɩ̃ a pʋ̃pãanyã? A bomo ala baarfʋ daar ɩn kũu.
45006022	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, Nãaŋmɩn na ben faa yɩ yin a yelbier pɔ a yɩ ɩ a wʋ gbãgbaar, a tɔ̃nɔ̃ yɩn nyɛ ɩn chɛchɛ ɩfʋ ka a baaraa ɩ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
45006023	Bojũu yelbier sãyar ɩn kũu, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ ɩ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ.
45007001	Yaa be bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, yɛɛr, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ a bala na bɔ̃ɔ a nɛbinãa ɩka a nɛbinãa ma tʋ̃ɔn nɩrɛ na chɛnɛ nɩ nɩbir ɛ?
45007002	De man pɔɔ na kul sɩrɛ, a nɛɛ lũ wʋn mar a sɩrɛ ka wʋ chire dayuo na gãn wʋ, a sɩrɛ na chɛnɛ ba kpi ɛ, tɩchɛ a sɩrɛ wa kpi, a kul taa nɛɛ 'lɔ ba lɛ lũ wʋ go ɛ.
45007003	'Lɔ wa tɩ ir dayuo a sɩrɛ na chɛnɛ vʋrɔ, ban 'yɛr naa ɩka wʋ sɔ̃ɔ naa. Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a sɩrɛ kpi naa, a nɛɛ ba lɛ lũ wʋ go ɛ, ala ɩ wʋ gba na kul dayuo, waa sɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
45007004	Lɛ lɛ, n yɛɛr yɩ mɩ kpin kʋ a nɛbinãa tu a Kɩrɩsɩto ɩ̃gãn pɔ, ka yɩn be be kʋ nɩyuo, a 'lɔ na ir a kũu pɔ ka sɩn tʋ̃ɔ wɔ̃ wɔ̃mɔ̃ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn.
45007005	Bojũu a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a yelbier ɩ̃gãn na so sɩ, ka a yelbier vɔlaa ma de a nɛbinãa tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ a sɩ ɩ̃gãn pɔ a sɩ wɔ̃nɔ̃ kũu wɔ̃mɔ̃.
45007006	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ kpin kʋ a 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ lũ sɩ, sɩ son sɩ mɩ̃ɛ yi a nɛbinãa 'lɔ pɔ, na sɩ pãa tʋ̃nɔ̃ a sɔpaalaa nyã pɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na ba ɩ a sɔkoraa ban sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ a gãn pɔ ɛ.
45007007	Bo lɛ sɩn lɛ 'yɛr go? A nɛbinãa ɩn yeldɛɛr bɩɩ? Kai, sɔr ba be be ɛ! Waa ɩ yeldɛɛr ɛ. Sɩrɛ jaa n kʋ̃ naa bɔ̃ɔ yelbier ɛ, ala ɩ a nɛbinãa ba be be ɛ. Bojũu n kʋ̃ naa bɔ̃ɔ jɩɛlfʋ ɛ, ala ɩ a nɛbinãa ba ta 'yɛr ɩka, "Taa jɩɛlɛ nɩrɛ bon ɛ."
45007008	Tɩchɛ a yelbier far kpɛ na wʋ nyɛ sɔr a nɛbinãa sɛ̃ vɛ̃ ka n wɔ̃ jɩɛlfʋ jaa bʋrɔ vɔlaa. A nɛbinãa baa be be ɛ, yelbier ɩn bʋ̃kũu.
45007009	Ɩn dɔ̃ɔ be be ba bɔ̃ɔ a nɛbinãa ɛ, tɩchɛ a nɛbinãa na wa wa, yelbier faan a nyɛvʋr, ka a kũu kʋ ma.
45007010	Be lɛ n nyɛ ɩka a nɛbinãa 'lɔ naa waan nyɛvʋr, kũu lɛ wʋ bar tɩ waan.
45007011	Bojũu a yelbier nyɛn sɔr a nɛbinãa na kʋ wʋ, a wʋ far kpɛ na wʋ bɛl ma, ka a tu a nɛbinãa nyã pɔ, ka a kũu kʋ ma.
45007012	A lɛ jũu, a nɛbinãa ɩn chɛchɛ, ka a nɛbinãa 'yɛr mɩ ɩ chɛchɛ, naa tor ɩ vɩla.
45007013	Bon 'lɔ na ɩ bʋ̃vɩla pãa lɩɛb kũu wa kʋ ma? A ba ɩ lɛ lɛ ɛ. Tɩchɛ n bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a ɩn yelbier, na a lɩɛb kũu kʋ ma tu a bon 'lɔ na ɩ vɩla pɔ. A tu naa 'yɛr binãa pɔ, ka bier na ɩ yelbier sɩrɛ jaa.
45007014	Sɩn bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a nɛbinãa ɩn Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ bon lɛ, tɩchɛ ka a maa ɩ ɩ̃gãn yelbier na da ka n ɩ a wʋ gbãgbaa.
45007015	N maa bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ ɩn maala ɛ, bojũu a ala ɩn bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maal n maa maal ɛ, tɩchɛ a ala ɩn 'laar lɛ n ma maala.
45007016	Ala ɩ n ma maala naa ala ɩn ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maala ɛ, n sɔɔ naa ɩka a nɛbinãa ɩn vɩla.
45007017	An ben be a lɛ, a ba ɩ maa mɩ̃ɛ lɛ bɔ̃ɔn tɩ ɩrɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yelbier 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na be a n pɔ lɛ ɩrɛ.
45007018	N bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka yelvɩla jaa ba be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a maa yelbier ɩ̃gãn tɛɛ lɛ. Bojũu n ma bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n maal vɩla tɩ naa maa tʋ̃ɔ maal ɛ.
45007019	Bojũu a ala ɩn maala ba ɩ a vɩla ala ɩn bʋɔrɔ a maalfʋ ɛ. Kai, a bier ala ɩn ba bʋɔrɔ a maalfʋ lɛ, ala lɛ n ma maala.
45007020	Pʋ̃pãanyã, ala ɩ n maala naa a ala ɩn ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maal ɛ, a ba lɛ ɩ maa lɛ lɛ maala go ɛ, tɩchɛ a yelbier 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na be a n 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ maala.
45007021	Lɛ lɛ, n nyɛn a lɛ a nɛbinãa na tʋ̃nɔ̃, maa wa bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maal vɩla, a yelbier lɛ ma tɔɔ gbʋr ma jaa yɛ̃ yɛ̃.
45007022	N bʋɔrɔ naa Nãaŋmɩn nɛbinãa nɩ a n pʋɔ wʋ jaa,
45007023	tɩchɛ n nyɛ naa a nɛbinãa ɩ̃sʋɔ na tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a n ɩ̃gãn jiir amɩne. Wʋ jɛɛrɛ nɩ naa a n tɩɛr na wʋ maal ma ka n ɩ a yelbier nɩpɔɔraa a n ɩ̃gãn jiir pɔ.
45007024	Nɩjarma lɛ n pãa ɩ! An lɛ na faa ma yin a yelbier ɩ̃gãn nyã na chiine ma a kũu jie?
45007025	Nãaŋmɩn son puorfʋ tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ! A maa mɩ̃ɛ a n tɩɛr pɔ, n ɩn a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ gbãgbaa, tɩchɛ a n yelbier ɩ̃gãn mɩ ɩ gbãgbaa kʋ a yelbier nɛɛ.
45008001	A lɛ jũu pʋ̃pãanyã, yele ba pɔɔrɔ a bala na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
45008002	A tun a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ jũu, a nɛɛ 'lɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nyɛvʋr faa man yin a nɛɛ 'lɔ na ɩ yelbier nɩ kũu pɔ.
45008003	Bojũu a bon 'lɔ a Mosesɩ nɛɛ na ba dɔ̃ɔ tara kpɛ̃ɔ na maal ɛ, a sɩ yelbier ɩ̃gãn na bal bar, Nãaŋmɩn maal naa na wʋ tʋ̃ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ Bie a wʋ nyɛtãan a sɩn na maala a yelbier kaar a wʋ wa ɩ a yelbier bɔɔrlo bon. Lɛ lɛ wʋ sɔ̃ɔ yelbier a nɩsaal pɔ bar,
45008004	ka a lɛ a Mosesɩ nɛbinãa na bʋɔrɔ ka a sɛɛ a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, a sɩ kʋ̃ lɛ turo a lɛ a yelbier ɩ̃gãn na bʋɔrɔ ɛ, tɩ turo a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na bʋɔrɔ.
45008005	A bala na turo a ba yelbier ɩ̃gãn, ba den a ba tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a ala na ɩ a ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa pɔ, tɩchɛ a bala mɩ na turo a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na bʋɔrɔ, mɩ den a ba tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a ala a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na bʋɔrɔ.
45008006	Yelbier sʋɔ tɩɛr ɩn kũu, tɩchɛ a tɩɛr 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na so ɩn nyɛvʋr nɩ nyã'maar.
45008007	A yelbe-ɩrɛ tɩɛr ma 'laar Nãaŋmɩn, wʋ maa siir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ ɛ, wʋ mɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ ɛ.
45008008	Bala na turo a lɛ a ba ɩ̃gãn na bʋɔrɔ, kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ pɛl Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ ɛ.
45008009	Yɩn 'lɔ ba lɛ turo a lɛ a yelbier ɩ̃gãn na bʋɔrɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ turo naa a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na bʋɔrɔ, ala ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ben a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ. Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba wa tara a Kɩrɩsɩto Sɩɛ ɛ, waa ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto tʋɔr ɛ.
45008010	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ Kɩrɩsɩto ben a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, a yɩ ɩ̃gãn kpi naa a yelbier jũu, tɩchɛ ka a yɩ sɩɩr tara nyɛvʋr a yeltorsɩ jũu.
45008011	Ala ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'lɔ na sɩ̃ɩ a Yesu a kũu pɔ, ben a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, 'lɔ na sɩ̃ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto a kũu pɔ, na kʋn a yɩ ɩ̃gãn kũn nyɛvʋr tu a wʋ Sɩɛ pɔ, a 'lɔ na be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
45008012	A lɛ jũu n yɛɛr, sɩ din sãn, tɩchɛ a ba ɩ a sɩ yelbier ɩ̃gãn nyã lɛ ɛ, a sɩn turo a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ ɛ.
45008013	Bojũu ala ɩ yɩ turo naa a lɛ a yɩ yelbier ɩ̃gãn na bʋɔrɔ, yɩn kpi naa, tɩchɛ ala ɩ yɩ den a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋ̃n a ɩ̃gãn ma maal bidɛbɛ bar, yɩ ben a nyɛvʋr sɔr pɔ.
45008014	Bojũu bala jaa a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na chiine, bala lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir.
45008015	A ba ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wʋn kʋ yɩ, waa maala yɩ gbãgbaar ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kʋrɔ yɩ go ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ kʋ yɩn a wʋ Sɩɛ a yɩ lɩɛb a wʋ bibiir. A Sɩɛ nyã lɛ sɩ ma de bʋɔlɔ wʋ, "N Sãa Nãaŋmɩn."
45008016	A Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ mɩ̃ɛ din dãasɩɛ nɩ a sɩ sɩɩr ɩka sɩ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn bibiir.
45008017	Pʋ̃pãanyã, ala ɩ sɩ ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn bibiir, sɩn lɛ so a bʋ̃sʋ̃n ala a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ, 'matãan a Kɩrɩsɩto. Ala ɩ sɩrɛ jaa, sɩ lɔ̃ɔn wʋn di a wʋ dɔɔyɛ, lɛ lɛ sɩ mɩn 'matãan wʋ põ a wʋ tɩɩr.
45008018	N man nyɛ a sɩ dɩna dɔɔyɛ ka waa jɩ̃ bon ɛ, ɩn de man a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr 'lɔ na wa nyɩr a sɩ sɛ̃.
45008019	A bʋ̃maalsɩ a jaa nyʋnyʋlɔ naa chɩlɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir wʋn wa vɛ̃ a ba nyɩrɛ.
45008020	Bojũu a bʋ̃maalsɩ a jaa ben a ɩ̃gãn sal pĩlem an ba ɩ a ba mɩ̃ɛ bɔfʋ ɛ,
45008021	tɩ ɩ a 'lɔ na maal ba bɔfʋ, na wʋ chɛnɛ tara ba nɩ tɩɛr sʋ̃, ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn na wa faa ban yin a gbãgbaa 'lɔ na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ kpɛ a mɩ̃ɛ sofʋ 'lɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir tɩɩr pɔ.
45008022	Bojũu sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa a bʋ̃maalsɩ a jaa na hʋ̃nɔ̃, ka a ɔɔrɔ ba fɩka pɔɔ na dɔɔrɔ yi a lɛ daar jaa wa tãn a dɩna.
45008023	A ba ɩ lɛ tɛɛ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a sɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋfʋ bidɔ̃ɔ, mɩ ʋrɔ a sɩ pʋɔm na sɩ nyʋnyʋlɔ chɛlɛ nɩ wʋn wa lɩɛb sɩ a wʋ bibiir, nɩ a faafʋ wʋn wa faan a sɩ ɩ̃gãma.
45008024	A tɩɛrtɔ nyãna jũu lɛ sɩ nyɛn a faafʋ. Tɩchɛ bon fʋn nyɛn nɩbir, fʋ maa lɛ tara a wʋ tɩɛr go ɛ. An lɛ ma tɩɛrɛ bon wʋn tara baar?
45008025	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ sɩ tɩɛrɛ na bon sɩn ba tara sɛrɛ ɛ, sɩ ma din kãnyir chɛlɛ.
45008026	A lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ma sʋ̃nɔ̃ sɩ a sɩ balfʋ pɔ. Saa bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ sɩn taa ma sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ mɩ̃ɛ lɛ ma de hʋ̃ʋnfʋ 'lɔ sɩn kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ man a 'yɛrbie ɛ, na wʋ ma sʋɔrɔ kʋrɔ sɩ.
45008027	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ma chɛl a sɩ nyãa bɔ̃ɔn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ tɩɛr, bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nyãna lɛ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ a wʋ nɩbɛ nɩ a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ.
45008028	Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a yele a jaa pɔ, Nãaŋmɩn ma tʋ̃n ka a ɩ sʋ̃ kʋ a bala na nʋ̃ wʋ, a bala wʋn tu a wʋ tɩɛr pɔ bʋɔl.
45008029	Bojũu bala a Nãaŋmɩn na de nie bɔ̃ɔn na wʋ chɛl ir ka ba lɩɛb kaara a wʋ Bie kaar, ka wʋn ɩ a yɛɛr ba jaa pɔ Bidadɔ̃ɔ.
45008030	A bala wʋn de nie ir, bala lɛ wʋ bʋɔl, a bala wʋn bʋɔl, bala lɛ wʋ vɛ̃ ka a ba yele tor, a bala mɩ wʋn vɛ̃ ka a ba yele tor, bala mɩ lɛ wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ tɩɩr.
45008031	Bo lɛ sɩn pãa 'yɛr nɩ a yele nyãna? Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn ben a sɩ sɛ̃, an lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ jɛb sɩ?
45008032	A 'lɔ na ba mɔ̃ɔ sɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ bie ɛ, tɩchɛ na wʋ sɔɔ bar sɔr ka ba kʋ wʋ a sɩ jũu, bo lɛ na ŋmaa wʋ sɔr ka wʋ kʋ̃ de a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ 'matãan a bomo a jaa kʋ sɩ ɛ?
45008033	An lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr 'yɛr dɔɔl a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na ir? Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ maal ba a ba tor.
45008034	An 'lɔ lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba 'yɛr? Nɩrɛ jaa ba be be ɛ. A Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nyã na kpi, 'lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn mɩ sɩ̃ɩ ka wʋ ir ɩ vʋr na wʋ ara Nãaŋmɩn nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, 'lɔ lɛ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ sɩ.
45008035	An lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ tɔɔ sɩ yin a Kɩrɩsɩto nʋ̃fʋ nyã pɔ? Wõm, bɩɩ wʋʋr, bɩɩ gefʋ, bɩɩ kɔ̃, bɩɩ sal'mʋɔr, bɩɩ dɔɔyɛ, bɩɩ ban na kʋ sɩ nɩ sʋɔ?
45008036	Nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "A yɩ jũu, sɩ ma tuor kũu bɩbir jaa. Ba ma kaa sɩn fɩka piir ban chiine nɩ kɔkɔɛ ŋmafʋ jie."
45008037	Kai, a anyãna a jaa pɔ, sɩ ɩ naa tʋ̃tʋ̃ɔnbɔ tu a 'lɔ na nʋ̃ sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
45008038	Bojũu n bɔ̃ɔn sɩrɛ jaa ɩka kũu, bɩɩ nyɛvʋr, bɩɩ malakasɩ, bɩɩ a sɩdɛbɛ, bɩɩ ka dɩna lɛ, bɩɩ nɩdaar, bɩɩ ka kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme lɛ,
45008039	ka dofʋ lɛ, bɩɩ suufʋ lɛ, bɩɩ bon jaa na be a bʋ̃maalsɩ pɔ lɛ, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tɔɔ sɩ yin a nʋ̃fʋ a Nãaŋmɩn na nʋ̃ sɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
45009001	Yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, n ba ŋmara jirsɩ ɛ, a n tɩɛr mɩ din dãasɩɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pɔ.
45009002	Nɩbaal kpɛ man tɩ põn bar, ka wʋʋr sɛɛ ma a nyãa.
45009003	An taa nʋ̃mɔ̃ ma naa ɩka n ben pɔ'yɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ naa ba lɛ pʋɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ ɛ, a n yɛɛr Isɩral nɩbɛ jũu, bala lɛ ɩ a n mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ.
45009004	A Isɩral nɩbɛ bala lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn de ka ba ɩ a wʋ bibiir, na wʋ kʋ ba a wʋ tɩɩr nɩ a nɛtɩrsɩ wʋn pɔn ba, na wʋ kʋ ba a nɛbinãa, nɩ a lɛ ban na puoro wʋ a wʋ puorfʋ yir nɩ a nɛɛr wʋn tɩr kʋ ba.
45009005	Bala lɛ ɩ a sãakpãmɩne, a ba pɔ lɛ ba bɩɛr a Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ na ɩ a nɩsaal yi, na wʋ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn kaara a bomo a jaa, 'lɔ lɛ ban pɛɛrɛ bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
45009006	A ba ɩ fɩka a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɩn faa ɛ, bojũu a ba ɩ a bala jaa ban dɔɔ a Isɩral nɩbɛ pɔ, ba jaa lɛ ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ɛ.
45009007	A ba ɩ baa yi a wʋ par pɔ ɛ, ba jaa baa ɩ Abraham bibiir ɛ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr nɛɛ kʋ a Abraham ɩka, "Isaakɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a fʋ yɔn na yi."
45009008	A ba ɩ a ɩ̃gãn vaar bibiir lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir ɛ, tɩchɛ a bibiir bala a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ a wʋ dɔɔ, bala lɛ wʋ kaa a ba ɩ Abraham bibiir.
45009009	Bojũu nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ 'yɛr, "A daar wa ta, ɩn lɩɛb wa ka a Saara dɔɔ dabile."
45009010	A ba ɩ anyã tɛɛ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a Worbɛka dɔɔn dabil ayi ka ba sãa ɩ bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ na ɩ a sɩ sãakpã Isaakɩ.
45009011	Sɛrɛ tɩ ka wʋ wa dɔɔ a yɩbɛ banyãna, baa mɩ maal yele jaa vɩla bɩɩ dɛɛr ɛ, tɩ nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a ɩ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ pɔ lɛ wʋ ma tu ir a nɩrɛ.
45009012	A kʋ̃ ɩ a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ jũu ɛ, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na bʋɔl fʋ. Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ a Worbɛka, "A yɛkarma na tʋ̃nɔ̃ na kʋrɔ a yɛbile."
45009013	Lɛ mɩ lɛ a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "N nʋ̃n Jekɔb tɩchɛ naa 'laar a Esau."
45009014	Bo lɛ sɩn pãa lɛ 'yɛr? Nãaŋmɩn ɩn nɩfɩlefɩle bɩɩ? Kai. Sɔr ba be be ɛ!
45009015	Bojũu wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Mosesɩ, "Nɩrɛ 'lɔ ɩn na kaa nɩbaal lɛ ɩn na kaa nɩbaal, naa maal vɩla kʋ a 'lɔ ɩn na maal vɩla kʋ."
45009016	A lɛ jũu a ba ɩ lɛ nɩrɛ na bʋɔrɔ ɛ, bɩɩ na tʋ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yin Nãaŋmɩn nɩbaal kaafʋ pɔ.
45009017	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a Ijipitɩ nãa Faaro ɩka yaa, "Maa lɛ bin fʋ a yele nyãna jũu, ɩka n wiil a n kpɛ̃ɔ a fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka ban bʋɔl a n yuor a wɛr wʋ jaa."
45009018	A lɛ jũu, Nãaŋmɩn ma kãan nɩrɛ 'lɔ wʋn bʋɔrɔ nɩbaal, a 'lɔ wʋ mɩn bʋɔrɔ, wʋ ma vɛ̃n ka a wʋ nyãa kpɛ̃mɛ.
45009019	Ɩ̃sʋɔ na sʋʋr ma naa ɩka, "Bo lɛ so ka a Nãaŋmɩn na de yele dɔɔl sɩ? Bojũu nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ tɔr a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ ɛ?"
45009020	Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ mɩ nɩ ana, nɩsaal na fʋn 'yɛr lɩɛr Nãaŋmɩn? "Laa na tʋ̃ɔn sʋʋr a 'lɔ na mɛ wʋ ɩka, 'Bo lɛ fʋ mɛ ma a nɩtɔ̃ ɔ?' "
45009021	A lamɩɛrɛ ba tara sɔr ɩka wʋ de a yɔɔr bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ mɛn bʋ̃ʋdʋʋ tɩchɛ mɛn ladiraa ɛ?
45009022	Bo lɛ, ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kaa ir ɩka wʋ wiil a wʋ suur na wʋ vɛ̃ a ba bɔ̃ɔn a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ, tɩ na wʋ chɛnɛ tara kãnyir nɩ a bonsɩ ala wʋn chɔɔr gun a sɔ̃ɔ barfʋ?
45009023	Bo lɛ, ala ɩ wʋ maal a nɩtɔ̃ ɩka a bonsɩ ala na ɩ a wʋ nɩbaal bomo, ka a bɔ̃ɔn a wʋ tɩɩr tɔ̃nɔ̃, a bala wʋn de nie chɔɔr gun a wʋ tɩɩr,
45009024	a sɩn gba wʋ mɩ na bʋɔl, na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ na wʋ bʋɔl a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ mɩ?
45009025	Nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ ka a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrɛ Hosea sɛb a wʋ gãn pɔ, "Ɩn bʋɔl ban a maa nɩbɛ, a bala na ba ɩ a n nɩbɛ ɛ, naa bʋɔl wʋ a n nɩ nʋ̃ naa, 'lɔ na ba dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a n nɩ nʋ̃ naa ɛ."
45009026	Ka wʋ sɛb a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ an ɩ a jie 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ wʋn 'yɛr ɩka, "Yaa ɩ a n nɩbɛ ɛ, bala naa lɛ ban lɛ bʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn vʋr bibiir."
45009027	Isaiya mɩ dɔ̃ɔ mʋɔl a Isɩral nɩbɛ na wʋ 'yɛr, "Ala ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ gba waan fɩka man nɛɛ bire, a bɩ̃lãa bala na wa chɛ, lɛ na nyɛ faafʋ.
45009028	Bojũu a sɩ Soro na pɔɔn naa a wʋ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ na wʋ ŋmaa a ju."
45009029	Isaiya dɔ̃ɔn de nie 'yɛr, "Ala ba ɩ a sɩ Soro na ɩ a gãdaa jaa gãdaa sʋɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ bar a sɩ par ŋmaa ɛ, sɩn taa mɩ nyʋɔl kaara a Sodom nɩ a Gomora tẽn kaar."
45009030	Bo lɛ sɩn pãa lɛ 'yɛr? A bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, na ba dɔ̃ɔ turo a yeltorsɩ ɛ, bala lɛ be tara yaa. A ba yele tor naa ban tara sɔɔfʋ jũu.
45009031	Tɩchɛ a Isɩral nɩbɛ na turo a yeltorsɩ ba tara yaa ɛ,
45009032	Bo lɛ so? Bojũu baa turo nɩ sɔɔfʋ ɛ, tɩ turo nɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃, na ba bãr a kʋsɩr bãraa.
45009033	Nɩtãa lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ a wʋ 'yɛr, "Nyɛ, n bin a kʋsɩr be a Jiyon ka nɩbɛ na bãra nɩ a pie 'lɔ na vɛ̃ ka ba loro, ka nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de wʋ, vɩ̃ kʋ̃ kpɛ wʋ ɛ."
45010001	N yɛɛr, lɛ a n nyãa na bʋɔrɔ ka n sʋɔrɔ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ɩka, a Isɩral nɩbɛ ba nyɛ faafʋ.
45010002	Bojũu ɩn tʋ̃ɔn di a ba dãasɩɛ ɩka ba tara na nɩbijɩɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn yele, tɩchɛ bɔ̃ɔfʋ lɛ ba pʋɔ a ba nɩbijɩɛ pɔ ɛ.
45010003	Ban ba bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn yeltorsɩ ɛ, tɩ na ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba bin a ba mɩ̃ɛ yeltorsɩ, baa siir ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn yeltorsɩ ɛ.
45010004	Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ ɩ a nɛbinãa tɛɛfʋ jie, ka nɩrɛ jaa na sɔɔ de wʋ, wʋn vɛ̃n ka a nɩnyɩnɛ yele tor.
45010005	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Mosesɩ man a lɛ a nɛbinãa na ma vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ yele tor, "A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na maala a lɛ a nɛbinãa na 'yɛr, na tara na nyɛvʋr."
45010006	Tɩchɛ a yeltorsɩ ala na yire a sɔɔfʋ pɔ 'yɛr naa, "Ta tɩɛr a fʋ nyãa pɔ sʋʋr ɩka, 'An lɛ na do a saaju?' Ka a lɛ wiil ɩka, tɩ tara a Kɩrɩsɩto suu waan.
45010007	Bɩɩ sʋʋr a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɩka, 'An lɛ na chen a kpĩi tẽe?' " Ka a lɛ wiil ɩka, tɩ ir a Kɩrɩsɩto a kũu pɔ waan.
45010008	Tɩchɛ bo lɛ a 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ? "A 'yɛr gbʋr fʋ naa, a ben a fʋ nɛɛ pɔ, naa be a fʋ nyãa pɔ." Ala lɛ ɩ a sɔɔfʋ 'yɛr nyã sɩn mʋɔlɔ.
45010009	Ala ɩ fʋ haan a fʋ nɛɛ chiir a fʋ pʋɔ 'yɛr ɩka, "A Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ ɩ a Soro," na fʋ sɔɔn a fʋ nyãa wʋ jaa ɩka, Nãaŋmɩn ir wʋn a kũu pɔ, fʋn nyɛn faafʋ.
45010010	Bojũu a fʋ nyãa 'lɔ fʋn sɔɔ den lɛ na vɛ̃ ka a fʋ yele tor, ka a fʋ nɛɛ 'lɔ fʋn haan 'yɛr lɛ na faafʋ.
45010011	Nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de wʋ, vɩ̃ kʋ̃ kpɛ wʋ ɛ."
45010012	Bojũu tɛɛ taa ba be a Juu nɩrɛ nɩ a 'lɔ na ba ɩ a Juu nɩrɛ ɛ. A Soro bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ɩ ba jaa Soro, na wʋ sʋ̃nɔ̃ a bala jaa na bʋɔlɔ a wʋ yuor.
45010013	Bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Bala jaa na bʋɔlɔ a Soro yuor ɩka wʋ sʋ̃ʋ ba, na nyɛn faafʋ."
45010014	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ban ɩrɛ wa bʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ ban ba sɔɔ ɛ? Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ban ɩ wa sɔɔ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ ban ba wõ a wʋ 'yɛr ɛ? Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ban ɩrɛ wa wõ a wʋ 'yɛr ka nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ ba wa mʋɔl a wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba ɛ?
45010015	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ ban ɩrɛ wa mʋɔl ka baa tʋ̃ ba ɛ? Nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Nyɛ lɛ a bala na waara nɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ gbɛɛ na vɩɛlɛ ka."
45010016	Tɩchɛ a ba ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ba jaa lɛ lɩɛb kaa a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã ɛ. Bojũu Isaiya dɔ̃ɔ sʋʋr, "Sɩ Soro, an lɛ sɔɔ de a sɩ 'yɛr?"
45010017	Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ ɩka 'yɛr fʋn ma wõ pɔ lɛ fʋ ma sɔɔ, ka a 'yɛrbie ala ban wõ ɩn a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr.
45010018	Tɩchɛ ka n sʋʋr, a mɔ̃ baa wõ naa ɛ? Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ ba wõ naa naa. "A ba kɔkɔr yin de jie wʋ jaa, ka a ba 'yɛr tɩ ta a wɛr tɛɛfʋ jie."
45010019	N lɛ sʋʋr kaa go, a mɔ̃ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ? Mosesɩ dɔ̃ɔ de nie 'yɛr, "A bala na ba ɩ paal ɛ, ɩn maal ba naa ka nyuur kpɛ yɩ, naa lɛ maal a paal 'lɔ na ba bɔ̃ɔ bon jaa ɛ, ka suur kpɛ yi."
45010020	Ka Isaiya mɩ ba dɔ̃ɔ jo dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩ 'yɛr ɩka, "A bala na ba dɔ̃ɔ yʋɔrɔ bʋɔrɔ ma ɛ, ba nyɛ ma naa, n wiil naa n mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a bala na ba dɔ̃ɔ sʋrɔ ma ɛ."
45010021	Tɩchɛ a Isɩral nɩbɛ 'lɔ, nɩtɔ̃ lɛ wʋ 'yɛr, "Bɩbir jaa lɛ n ma tur a n nuur bʋɔlɔ a bibawõnsɩ nɩ a nɩdɛbɛ, na turo a sɔɩ ala na ba vɩɛlɛ ɛ bʋɔrɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ tɩɛrsɩ bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ."
45011001	N pãa sʋʋr naa, a Nãaŋmɩn ben tɔr a wʋ nɩbɛ bar bɩɩ? Kai! A maa mɩ̃ɛ ɩn a Isɩral nɩrɛ, naa ɩ a Abraham yɔ̃ɔ yi a Benjamin bʋrɔ pɔ.
45011002	Nãaŋmɩn ba tɔr a wʋ nɩbɛ bar ɛ, bala lɛ wʋ de nie bɔ̃ɔ. Yaa bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr, lɛ a Elaija na dɔ̃ɔ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn waala dɔɔlɔ a Isɩral nɩbɛ,
45011003	"N Soro, ba kʋn a fʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ, na ba wɛl a fʋ bɔɔr lofʋ jiir bar. Maa tɛɛ lɛ chɛ, tɩ a ba bʋɔrɔ a n kʋfʋ."
45011004	Bo lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ a Elaija? Wʋ 'yɛr naa, "N chɛnɛ na tara nɩbɛ tur ata kɔɔr anũu (7,000) na ba gbur dumo puor a tɩɩ Baal ɛ."
45011005	Lɛ mɩ lɛ a dɩna, nɩbɛ bamɩne chɛ naa ka Nãaŋmɩn na ir ba a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu.
45011006	Ala be ɩ a wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu lɛ, a ba lɛ ɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ go ɛ, ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, a wɩ̃ɛfʋ kʋ̃ lɛ ɩ wɩ̃ɛfʋ lɛ go ɛ.
45011007	Bo pãa lɛ? A ala a Isɩral nɩbɛ na bʋɔrɔ nɩbijɩɛ baa nyɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na ir lɛ nyɛ. Ka a bala na chɛ kpɛ̃mɛ a ba nyãa.
45011008	Nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃n ka ba ɩ jaa bũrtũm wa tãn a dɩna. A ba nɩbie ala maa tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ bon ɛ, ka a ba tobo ala maa tʋ̃ɔ wõ 'yɛr ɛ."
45011009	A Nãa David mɩ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a ba 'yɛr a wʋ gãn pɔ, "Vɛ̃ ka a ba bʋ̃diir difʋ jie ka a lɩɛb bʋ̃nyɔɔrsɩ nɩ chɛɛr, ka a ɩ a ba bãr lofʋ jie nɩ a ba sãyar.
45011010	A ba nɩbie a jɔ̃ɔ, a ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ jaa ɛ, na ba kab gʋ̃mɔ̃ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ dɔl ɛ."
45011011	N lɛ sʋʋr go, ba ben bãr na lo na ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ir jaa ɛ? A ba ɩ lɛ ɛ. A ba maal bɔrfʋ jũu, a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, nyɛn faafʋ ka nyuur na kpɛ a Isɩral nɩbɛ.
45011012	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a ba maal bɔrfʋ vɛ̃n ka a wɛr wʋ jaa le, ka a ba bɔrfʋ mɩ le a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, a bala mɩ̃ɛ wa pʋɔ ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an kaara!
45011013	Yɩn na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ, an ben ɩka maa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn ir tʋ̃ a yɩ pɔ, ka n ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nãa a yɩn na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ pɔ. N mʋ̃ɔn nɩbir nɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ nyã.
45011014	A maa tɩɛr lɛ ɩka nyuur wʋ kpɛ a maa mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ ka n tʋ̃ɔ a bamɩne faa.
45011015	Bojũu ala ɩ a ba tɔr barfʋ ɩn 'maalfʋ kʋ a wɛr, ka a Nãaŋmɩn lɛ wa de ba, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an kaara, a kʋ̃ kaara fɩka nɩrɛ na yi kũu pɔ tara nyɛvʋr ɛ?
45011016	Ala ɩ fʋ den a paanʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, a paanʋ̃ɔ ala na chɛ, a jaa ɩn chɛchɛ. Ala ɩ fʋ den a tɩɛ nyɩɩr kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, a tɩɛ wilsɩ mɩ ɩn chɛchɛ.
45011017	Ala ɩ ba 'mɛl a tɩɛ mɩ̃ɛ wile ɩ̃sʋɔ bar tɩ ŋmaa a yɩn na ɩ a mʋɔ pɔ tɩɛ wile wa mar ka yɩ 'mataa tɔɔrɔ nyuro a kɔ̃bʋ̃'yen yire a tɩɛ ɩ̃gãn pɔ nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃,
45011018	taa tɩɛr ɩka fʋ sa naa a wilsɩ ala ɛ. Fʋ̃ʋ wa 'mɔɔrɔ fʋ mɩ̃ɛ, lɩɛb tɩɛr kaa ɩka a ba ɩ a fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ a wile lɛ tuo a nyɩbɛ ɛ, tɩ a nyɩbɛ lɛ tuo a fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ a wile.
45011019	Yɩn 'yɛr yɩn pãa na 'yɛr nɩ nyã, "Ba 'mɛl a wilsɩ ala bar tɩ pãa na de ma mar."
45011020	A lɛ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ, tɩchɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ 'mɛl ba bar a ba ba sɔɔfʋ jũu, tɩchɛ ka a yɩn ara nɩ sɔɔfʋ. Yɩ ta bʋɔrɔ yuor ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ.
45011021	Bojũu ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn ba dɔ̃ɔ bar a tɩɛ mɩ̃ɛ wilsɩ ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ bar a yɩn mɩ ɛ.
45011022	Yɩ tɩɛr kaa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a maal vɩla sʋɔ ka a wʋ yele mɩ kpɛ̃mɛ, a wʋ yele kpɛ̃mɛ na kʋ a bala na lo, tɩchɛ na wʋ maal vɩla kʋ a yɩn, ala ɩ yɩ chɛnɛ na chiine a wʋ maal vɩla pɔ. Ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, wʋn ŋmaa yɩn bar.
45011023	Ala wa ɩ ba tɛɛn a ba baal bar, Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ɔn de ba lɛ mar a tɩɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ, Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ɔn lɛ de ba mar a lɛ go.
45011024	Yɩ kaa, ala ɩ a yɩn ban ŋmaa yin a mʋɔ pɔ tɩɛ pɔ wa mar a yir tɩɛ ban sɛl, an lɛ ɩn tuo a yir tɩɛ wilsɩ ala ban dɔ̃ɔ 'mɛl bar marfʋ bɩɩ?
45011025	N ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka n vɛ̃ ka a yelsɔɔlaa nyã sɔɔl a yɩn na ɩ a n yɛɛr tɩ ba ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ɛ, ka yɩ taa bʋɔrɔ yuor nɩ a yele nyã ɛ. A Isɩral nɩbɛ tara na a nyãkpɩ̃ɛn a lɛ nɛ na tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a bala na ba ɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ɛ, na wa tɩ nyɛ a faafʋ baar.
45011026	Lɛ lɛ na ɩ tɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ ba jaa pãa nyɛ faafʋ nɩtãa lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Fafaara na yin be a Jiyon wa, na wʋ wa lɩɛb tɩɛr jaa na ba vɩɛlɛ ɛ, yin a Jekɔb bal nɩbɛ pɔ bar.
45011027	A nɛtɩraa lɛ a nyãna ɩn na tara nɩ ba, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn wa de a ba yeldɛbɛ a jaa bar."
45011028	Fʋ̃ʋ kaa, a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã vɛ̃n ka ba ɩ Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃dẽme a yɩn na sɔɔ de jũu. Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a irfʋ pɔ mɩ lɛ, bala lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃ yɔɔ a ba sãakpãmɩne jũu.
45011029	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ nɩ a wʋ bʋɔlfʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ lɩɛb jaa ɛ.
45011030	Nɩtãa lɛ a yɩn mɩ na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, na yaa dɔ̃ɔ wõnõ a Nãaŋmɩn toor ɛ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã yɩ nyɛn a wʋ nɩbaal a ba bawõfʋ jũu.
45011031	Lɛ lɛ a bala mɩ na ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ, ba mɩ lɩɛb ɩ bawõnsɩ, na ba pãa mɩ na nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbaal a pʋ̃pãanyã, nɩtãa lɛ a sɩn mɩ na nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbaal.
45011032	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn pɔɔn a nɩbɛ ba jaa a bawõnsɩ die pɔ, na wʋn tʋ̃ɔ kaa ba jaa nɩbaal.
45011033	Nyɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn lefʋ na suu jɩ̃. A wʋ yɛ̃ nɩ a wʋ bɔ̃ɔfʋ ba gbʋr ɛ! A wʋ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ ba be bɔ̃ɔfʋ ɛ. A wʋ sɔɩ mɩ ba be bɩɛrfʋ ɛ!
45011034	"An lɛ dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro tɩɛr? Bɩɩ an lɛ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a wʋ 'yɛr sʋ̃nɔ̃."
45011035	"An lɛ dɔ̃ɔ de nie kʋ Nãaŋmɩn bon, ka wʋ pãa wa yara a sãn?"
45011036	Bojũu wʋ jie lɛ a bomo a jaa yi. 'Lɔ lɛ maal a jaa, na wʋ so a bonsɩ a jaa. 'Lɔ lɛ so a tɩɩr bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
45012001	A lɛ jũu, n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa yɛɛr, a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbaal nyã jũu, yɩ de a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ na ɩ bʋ̃nɩbie lon bɔɔr kʋ Nãaŋmɩn. A ɩn chɛchɛ naa pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ. Lɛ lɛ ɩ a puorfʋ na tara par.
45012002	Yɩ taa lɛ wa lɩɛrɛ maala a lɛ a wɛr nɩbɛ na maala go ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ maala a lɛ na lɩɛrɛ yɩ a tɩɛr paalaa nyã yɩn nyɛ. Yɩn pãa tʋ̃ɔn bɛɛr na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ, a ala na ɩ vɩla naa pɛlɛ a wʋ pʋɔ naa ɩ chɛchɛ.
45012003	A Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ nyã wʋn wɩ̃ɛ ma jũu, n sʋɔrɔ naa a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ɩka, ta tɩɛr a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ tɩ põn bar a lɛ yɩn taa tɩɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ma tɩɛr a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ nɩbijɩɛ jaa jɩ̃ a sɔɔfʋ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ yɩ.
45012004	Nɩtãa lɛ a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na tara ɩ̃gãn tɩ ka a tara jidẽdẽme, a jidẽdẽme anyãna ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ tʋ̃bʋ̃'yen ɛ.
45012005	Lɛ mɩ lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ, a sɩn bala na ɩ yɔɔ tɩ lɔ̃ɔ ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen pɔ, a jidẽdẽme anyã a jaa 'mantaa tʋ̃nɔ̃.
45012006	Sɩ jaa tara na kʋfʋsɩ na tɛɛ taa, tu a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋn wɩ̃ɛn sɩ. Ala ɩ a ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋfʋ ɩn a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr 'yɛrfʋ lɛ, wʋ ma 'yɛrɛ jɩ̃ a lɛ a wʋ sɔɔfʋ na ta.
45012007	Ka ala ɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ tʋ̃fʋ mɩ lɛ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ ma tʋ̃nɔ̃, ala ɩ wiilfʋ mɩ lɛ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ ma wile.
45012008	Ala ɩ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ lɛ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ ma 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn. Ka ala ɩ a wʋ kʋfʋ lɛ nɩbaalsɩ sʋ̃ʋfʋ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ ma sʋ̃nɔ̃ ba nɩ pʋpɛl. Ala ɩ nɩdiere tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ, vɛ̃ a wʋ ma mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃. Ala wa ɩ nɩbɛ 'maalfʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ, wʋ ma maala a lɛ nɩ chɩlfʋ.
45012009	Nʋ̃fʋ wʋ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ nʋ̃fʋ. 'Laar bon 'lɔ na ɩ dɛɛr, tɩ 'mar bon 'lɔ na ɩ sʋ̃.
45012010	Yɩ chɛlɛ taa yele, na yɩ de a yɛɛr nʋ̃fʋ nʋ̃n taa. Yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yɩ taaba gar a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ.
45012011	Yɩ ta ɩ nɩ tũtũlsɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ vɛ̃ ka a nʋ̃mɔ̃ yɩ a yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a sɩ Soro tʋ̃mɔ̃.
45012012	Yɩ chɩlɛ nɩ a yɩ tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie, na yɩ tara kãnyir a yɩ wõm pɔ, na yɩ tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a yɩ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ pɔ.
45012013	Yɩ ma lɔ̃ɔ põn a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ bala na ba tara bon jaa ɛ, na yɩ ma diere sãanba a yɩ yie pɔ.
45012014	Na yɩ 'yɛrɛ nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bala na gere yɩ, na yɩ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ ba, yɩ ta pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ ba ɛ.
45012015	Yɩ chɩlɛ nɩ a bala na chɩlɛ, na yɩ mɩ pʋɔ a bala na kõnõ na yɩ kõnõ.
45012016	A yɩn nɩ a bala na kpɩɛrɛ, yɩ tara tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen. Yɩ ta kaara ba pɔrɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ sɔɔ 'matãan a nɩbɛ bala na ba jɩ̃ yɩ ɛ. Yɩ ta kaa ɩka yɩn ɩn yɛ̃ dẽme ɛ.
45012017	Yɩ ta de bier yãan bier sãn ɛ. Yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, na yɩ maala a ala na vɩɛlɛ nɩrɛ jaa niem.
45012018	Ala ɩ an tʋ̃ɔ naa, an ɩ yɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ, yɩ tara nyã'maar nɩ a bala jaa yɩn lɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ nɩ.
45012019	N barmɩne, yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa yaara taa sãn ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ baraa kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn suur. Bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Maa lɛ so a sãn yaafʋ, ɩn lɩɛb yaa a sãn." Lɛ lɛ a Soro 'yɛr.
45012020	Lɛ an na ɩ lɛ ɩka, "Ala ɩ kɔ̃ kpɛ̃n a fʋ dɔ̃sʋɔ, kʋ wʋ bʋ̃diir a wʋ di. Ala ɩ kɔ̃nyũur wa kpɛ wʋ naa, kʋ wʋ kʋ̃ɔ a wʋ nyũ. Fʋ̃ʋ be maala a nɩtɔ̃, an kaara fɩka bũu saalbie lɛ fʋ mʋ̃ɔ dɔɔl wʋ a jum."
45012021	Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka bier tʋ̃ɔ yɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ de vɩla tʋ̃ɔn bier.
45013001	A yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ ma siir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a paal nɩbɛrɛ, bojũu kpɛ̃ɔ jaa ba be be ka a ba ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ bin ɛ. Kpɛ̃ɔ sʋɔ jaa ba be be ka Nãaŋmɩn ba lɛ bin wʋ ɛ.
45013002	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na chɩrɛ nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme ba nyãna, a Nãaŋmɩn na bin ba lɛ wʋ chɩrɛ nɩ, ka a bala na ɩrɛ a lɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔn ba mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr.
45013003	Bojũu a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme maa diere bier dɔɔlɔ a bala na maala vɩla ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala na maala a dɛɛr lɛ ba ma de yele dɔɔlɔ. Fʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka fʋ ta joro a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme dãbɩ̃ɛ bɩɩ? Fʋ pãa maala a lɛ na vɩɛlɛ, ban dãna fʋ naa.
45013004	Bojũu wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɩka wʋ maal fʋ vɩla. Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ wa maal dɛɛr 'lɔ, vɛ̃ ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kʋrɔ fʋ, a ba ɩ pɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ tara a sʋɔ ɛ. Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ lɛ wʋ ɩ na ara kʋ yeltorsɩ ɩka wʋ kpãana a bala na maala dɛɛr.
45013005	A lɛ jũu, a tara na sɔr ka yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, a ba ɩ ban na kpãa yɩ tɛɛ jũu ɛ, tɩchɛ an ɩ a yɩn mɩ̃ɛ mɩ bɔ̃ɔ nyɔɔfʋ jũu.
45013006	A anyãna jũu lɛ so yɩn yara lõpoo kʋrɔ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ na de a ba sɔ̃ɔ wʋ jaa tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ.
45013007	Nɩrɛ jaa sãn fʋn wa di, yab wʋ. Ka ala ɩ lõpoo lɛ faa yab ɛ, yab. Ka tẽmaal libie yabfʋ lɛ bɩɩ, yɩ ma yab, na yɩ joro a 'lɔ a jofʋ na sɛɛn, tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a 'lɔ mɩ a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ na sɛɛn.
45013008	Yɩ taa pɛ̃nɛ taa libie ka sãn ma gã a yɩ chara pɔ ɛ, a sãn 'lɔ tɛɛ na gã a yɩ chara pɔ lɛ, nʋ̃fʋ yɩn na nʋ̃ nʋ̃ taa, bojũu nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na nʋ̃ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ tun a lɛ a nɛbinãa na 'yɛr a jaa.
45013009	A 'yɛrbinsɩ lɛ a anyãna, "Ta sɛ̃ ɛ." "Ta kʋ nɩrɛ ɛ." "Ta ju nɩrɛ bon ɛ." "Ta jɩɛlɛ nɩrɛ bon ɛ." A 'yɛrbinsɩ ala a jaa nɩ pãa chɛ, ba den a jaa 'yɛr 'yɛr bir bʋ̃'yen ɩka, "Nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ nɩtãa a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ."
45013010	Fʋ̃ʋ wa nʋ̃ nɩrɛ, faa maala wʋ bier ɛ. Ala lɛ so, fʋ̃ʋ wa tara nʋ̃fʋ, fʋ tu naa a lɛ jaa a Mosesɩ nɛɛ na 'yɛr.
45013011	Yɩ maala a nɩtɔ̃, bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa lɛ a dɩna sɔ̃ɔ nyã na kaara. A sɔ̃ɔ ta naa ɩka yɩ jɛɔ ir a yɩ gʋ̃ɔ pɔ, bojũu a sɩ faafʋ gbʋr jaa yɛ̃yɛ̃ gar a bɩbir 'lɔ sɩn dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ de.
45013012	A chɛn bɩ̃lãa ka a tɩ̃sɔɔ baar, tɩchɛ ka a ɩ a wɛr mɩ tɔ̃ɔ chaar a lɛ nɛ. Yɩ ɩ a sɩ yaar a tɩ̃sɔɔ bomo bar tɩ de a chãa bomo su.
45013013	Yɩ ɩ a sɩ kpɩɛrɛ jaa kãkar fɩka a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩbɛ, na sɩ ir sɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin dɩ̃ɛn bɔyuor pɔ, dãa buufʋ pɔ, sɛ̃sɛ̃yele pɔ, nɩ folaa ɩfʋ pɔ, bɩɩ gɔ̃mɔ̃ bɔfʋ nɩ nyuur pɔ.
45013014	Tɩchɛ yɩ de a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na yɩ su pɔɔ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, na yɩ ta lɛ tɩɛrɛ ɩka yɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ a yɩ ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa na bʋɔrɔ go ɛ.
45014001	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ sɔɔfʋ na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ, yɩ ma sɔɔ de wʋ na yɩ ta tɔɔrɔ a wʋ yelbil 'yɛr ɛ.
45014002	Ɩ̃sʋɔ sɔɔfʋ ma vɛ̃n ka waa chire bon jaa ɛ, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ sɔɔfʋ mɩ na bal ka 'lɔ mɩ dire jɛvai tɛɛ.
45014003	A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba chire bon jaa ɛ, wʋ ta kaara a 'lɔ na ba dire a jaa pɔrɔ ɛ, a fʋ̃ʋ nyã mɩ na ba dire a jaa ɛ, ta kpɛrɛ a 'lɔ na dire a jaa ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn de wʋ naa.
45014004	Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ nɩ ana na fʋn tɔɔr nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ 'yɛr? A wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ sɛ̃ ka wʋ ara na bɩɩ wʋ lo naa, wʋn lɛ ara na, bojũu a wʋ Soro na tʋ̃ɔn maal wʋ a wʋ ara.
45014005	Nɩrɛ ma kãan a bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ a wʋ gar ɩ̃sʋɔ, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ kaa a bɩbie a jaa ka a ɩ bʋ̃'yen. Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ ma tɩɛr kaa a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩɛr pɔ.
45014006	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na de a bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ a wʋ gar a jaa, wʋ ɩrɛ a lɛ a sɩ Soro jũu. 'Lɔ na ɔɔrɔ a nʋ̃n, wʋ ɔɔrɔ a sɩ Soro jũu, bojũu wʋ ma sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ. A 'lɔ mɩ na ba ɔɔrɔ ɛ, wʋ mɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ a sɩ Soro jũu, wʋ mɩ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan.
45014007	Bojũu nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba be be kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɛɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ. Nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mɩ ba kpi kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɛɛ ɛ.
45014008	Ala ɩ sɩ ben ka, sɩ ben be kʋ a sɩ Soro. Ala ɩ sɩ mɩ kpi naa, sɩ kpin kʋ a sɩ Soro. Ka sɩ chɛnɛ na vʋrɔ, bɩɩ sɩ kpi naa, a sɩ Soro lɛ so sɩ.
45014009	A anyãna jũu lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto kpi tɩ na wʋ lɛ ir ɩ vʋr, ɩka a wʋ ɩ a kũn nɩ a vʋɛ ba jaa Soro.
45014010	Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ, baa 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ fʋ tɔɔrɔ a fʋ yɛbɛ 'yɛr, bɩɩ bo lɛ so ka fʋ kaara a fʋ yɛbɛ pɔrɔ? Bojũu sɩ jaa lɛ na ara a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ dakɔɔ par.
45014011	A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "A sɩ Soro lɛ 'yɛr, ɩn ɩ vʋr jũu, a gbɛdumo a jaa na gbur a n niem, ka a kɔkɔr jaa haa 'yɛr ɩka maa lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn."
45014012	Be lɛ a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na pãa 'yɛr a sɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn.
45014013	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ɩ a sɩ bar a sɩ taaba 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ, na sɩ lɩɛb a sɩ tɩɛr na sɩ ta ɩrɛ kʋsɩr bãraa kʋrɔ a sɩ taaba sɔɩ pɔ a ba ŋmiere loro ɛ.
45014014	A maa na be a sɩ Soro Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ, n sɔɔn sɩrɛ jaa ɩka bʋ̃diraa jaa ba ɩ dɛɛr a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa kãan bon ɩka wʋ ɩn bʋ̃dɛɛr, a bʋ̃nyɩnɛ ɩn bʋ̃dɛɛr kʋ wʋ.
45014015	Ala wa ɩ a chɛn a fʋ yɛbɛ bʋ̃diraa kɔ̃ɔ fʋn di jũu, faa maala wile nɩ nʋ̃fʋ ɛ. Ta vɛ̃ ka a fʋ bʋ̃dirsɩ sɔ̃ɔ a fʋ yɛbɛ 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto na kpi ɛ.
45014016	Ta vɛ̃ ka a bon 'lɔ fʋ̃ʋ na bʋɔlɔ bʋ̃vɩla, ka nɩrɛ bʋɔl wʋ bʋ̃dɛɛr ɛ.
45014017	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ yele ba ɩ bʋ̃diir nɩ bʋ̃nyursɩ yele ɛ, tɩchɛ a ɩn torfʋ, nɩ nyã'maar nɩ a pʋpɛl na yi a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pɔ yele lɛ,
45014018	bojũu nɩrɛ jaa na tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto tu a sɔr nyã pɔ, wʋ maala na a lɛ na pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ, ka a nɩbɛ mɩ 'yɛrɛ a nɩnyɩnɛ 'yɛr vɩla.
45014019	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ɩ a sɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir, na sɩ maala a lɛ na waan nyã'maar a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔn taa ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
45014020	Yɩ ta de bʋ̃diir yele sɔ̃ɔn a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃mɔ̃ bar ɛ. Bʋ̃diraa a jaa vɩɛlɛ naa, tɩchɛ a ɩn dɛɛr ala ɩ nɩrɛ din bon na vɛ̃ ka a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ lo.
45014021	A lɛ a sɛɛ naa ka nɩrɛ ta 'wɔb nʋ̃n ɛ, bɩɩ nyũ dãa ɛ, bɩɩ maal yele kɔ̃ɔ na vɛ̃ ka a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ lo ɛ.
45014022	Lɛ jaa fʋn bɔ̃ɔ a yelsɩ anyãna pɔ, bar ka a be a fʋ̃ʋ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn chara pɔ. Pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ tɩɛr na ba 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ yele nɩ a bonsɩ ala a 'lɔ mɩ̃ɛ na 'yɛr ɩka a ɩ naa ɛ.
45014023	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na dire nɩ baal, 'yɔ̃ɔn a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr, bojũu waa dire nɩ sɔɔfʋ ɛ. Bon jaa mɩ na ba wa yi sɔɔfʋ pɔ ɛ, a ɩn bier.
45015001	Sɩn bala na kpɛ̃mɛ, a sɛɛ naa ka sɩ tuo a bala na ba kpɛ̃mɛ ɛ, na loro tuor, na sɩ ta pɛlɛ a sɩn mɩ̃ɛ pʋʋr ɛ.
45015002	A sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ ma pɛlɛ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ pʋɔ, na sɩ sʋ̃ʋ wʋ a wʋ mɩ ba nyɩbɛ.
45015003	Bojũu a Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ̃ɛ gba mɩ ba dɔ̃ɔ pɛl a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ pʋɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ a lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "A tʋbie ala a bala na tʋfʋ, a wa dɔɔl a n ju."
45015004	Bojũu a ala a jaa na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, a kõr jaa bin, a sɛb a sɩn wiilfʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a gãma anyãna kʋ sɩ kãnyir 'yɔ̃ɔn sɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn ka sɩ tara tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie.
45015005	A Nãaŋmɩn na kʋrɔ yɩ a kãnyir na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ yɩ a ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn, wʋ kʋ yɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen ka yɩ turo nɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto.
45015006	Ka yɩ jaa 'mataa tara tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen na yɩ de nɛbʋ̃'yen 'yɔ̃ɔn a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr na ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto Sãa.
45015007	Yɩ sɔɔ diere taa nɩtãa lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ na sɔɔ de yɩ, ka yɩn tʋ̃ɔ waan pɛɛfʋ wa kʋ Nãaŋmɩn.
45015008	N 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a Kɩrɩsɩto wa lɩɛb naa a Juu nɩbɛ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ jũu, na wʋ vɛ̃ ka a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a sɩ Sãakpãmɩne ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
45015009	Ka a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, mɩ na tʋ̃ɔ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr a wʋ nɩbaal jũu. Nɩtãa lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "A lɛ jũu, ɩn dãnfʋ naa a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ sɛ̃, naa yiel yiel kʋ a fʋ yuor."
45015010	A lɛ sɛb go, "A yɩn na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, yɩ 'matãan a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ chɩlɛ."
45015011	A lɛ sɛb go, "A yɩn na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, yɩ pɛɛrɛ a sɩ Soro, na yɩ yiele pɛɛfʋ yiel kʋrɔ wʋ, a yɩn nɩbɛ ba jaa."
45015012	Isaiya gba mɩ lɛ 'yɛr go a wʋ gãn pɔ, "A Jesɩ nyɩɩr na lɛ tɔ naa. 'Lɔ lɛ na ir na wʋ kaara a paalsɩ a jaa, na wʋ mɩ ɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie."
45015013	A Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a yɩ tɩɛrtɔfʋ sʋɔ, wʋ sɛɛ a yɩ nyãn nɩ chɩlfʋ, nɩ nyã'maar a lɛ yɩn sɔɔ wʋ, ka a yɩ tɩɛrtɔfʋ pãa ŋme yaar nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ.
45015014	N yɛɛr, maa mɩ̃ɛ sɔɔ naa ɩka yɩ sɛɛn naa vɩla maalfʋ, na yɩ tara yɛ̃ na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ taa wiilfʋ.
45015015	N sɛb a da sɛɛr amɩne 'yɔ̃ɔ kʋ yɩ, ka a kaara fɩka n lɛ bɔ̃ɔ tɩɛr yɩ go, a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋn kʋ ma
45015016	ka n ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ naa tʋ̃nɔ̃ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ pɔ jũu, naa sʋ̃nɔ̃ mʋɔlɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ. Lɛ lɛ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, puorfʋ na tara par ka a Nãaŋmɩn sɔɔ de na wʋ oon ba nɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ.
45015017	Ɩn be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ jũu, a tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn yin yuor.
45015018	N kʋ̃ wa 'la 'yɛr 'yɛr jaa ɛ, ka a ala a Kɩrɩsɩto na maal baar ba lɛ ɛ, tu a n 'yɔ̃ɔ ka a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, lɩɛrɛ wa wõnõ a Nãaŋmɩn toor, tu a lɛ ɩn 'yɛr nɩ a lɛ ɩn tʋ̃,
45015019	wʋ den kpɛ̃ɔ tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ tʋ̃fɛrsɩ tun a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ. Lɛ lɛ, n yin a Jerusalɛm chen lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ gʋɔr a Ilirikum tẽe naa man a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna jaa nɛ nɛ nɛ.
45015020	Maa nɩbijɩɛ yele lɛ ɩka n mʋɔl 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ jie 'lɔ jaa ban ba wõ a Kɩrɩsɩto yele ɛ, naa ta ɩrɛ wa mɛ dɔɔl nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ dachin par kparaa ju ɛ.
45015021	Nɩtãa lɛ an dɔ̃ɔ sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "A bala ban ba dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ɛ, na nyɛ naa, ka a bala mɩ na ba dɔ̃ɔ wõ naa ɛ, na bɔ̃ɔn a par."
45015022	A yele nyãna lɛ var ma a sɔr ka n ba tʋɔrɔ waara a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ.
45015023	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ, n ba lɛ tara jipaalaa ka a paalsɩ anyã pɔ na lɛ tʋ̃ go ɛ, n mɩn dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔrɔ a yɩ nyɛfʋ a yuon yɔ̃ɔ na po jũu.
45015024	N guor naa ɩka n chen Sɩpẽen, maa wa tala ɩn ara na piir yɩ kaa, naa jɛ̃ a yɩ sɛ̃ bɩ̃lãa a yɩ sʋ̃ʋ ma ka n chen.
45015025	Pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ, Jerusalɛm lɛ n chiine nɩ a sʋ̃ʋfʋ ɩka n tɩ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo a be.
45015026	Bojũu a Masedonɩya dẽme nɩ a Akaya dẽme man taa ɩka ba chɩɛr chɩɛrfʋ sʋ̃ʋn a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo bamɩne na be a Jerusalɛm na ba tara bon jaa ɛ.
45015027	Ba nyɛn a lɛ ka a ɩ sãn kʋ ba a ba de a lɛ dɔɔl a ba mɩ̃ɛ. Ala ɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, põn naa a Juu nɩbɛ a Nãaŋmɩn sʋ̃ʋfʋsɩ, ala lɛ so ka a mɩ sɛɛ ɩka ba mɩ lɔ̃ɔn a Juu nɩbɛ põn a ba bʋ̃tarsɩ.
45015028	Maa wa tʋ̃ a nɩtɔ̃, naa de a chɩɛrfʋsɩ anyã kʋ ba baar, ala lɛ ɩn chen a Sɩpẽen naa tɩ 'lɔɔ piir yɩ kaa.
45015029	N bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka maa wa waara, ɩn waan naa a Kɩrɩsɩto sʋ̃ʋfʋ na bɛrma.
45015030	N sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa n yɛɛr, nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ nʋ̃fʋ ɩka, yɩ pʋɔ ma a n mɔ̃fʋ nyã pɔ, sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ ma.
45015031	Yɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn, a wʋ faa ma yin a bala na ba sɔɔ be a Judiya, ka a lɛ mɩ ɩn chiine a Jerusalɛm ka a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo mɩ tɩ sɔɔ de,
45015032	ka ala ɩka Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ lɛ, ka n wa a yɩ sɛ̃ nɩ pʋpɛl a sɩ 'mataa 'yɔ̃ɔ taa ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
45015033	Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a nyã'maar sʋɔ, wʋ be a yɩ jaa sɛ̃. A ɩ a lɛ.
45016001	N pʋrɔ naa a sɩ yɛpɔɔ Fiibi yovɩla kʋrɔ yɩ, a pɔɔ nyã ɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ be a Kenkɩrya tẽdẽme pupuorbiir pɔ.
45016002	N sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa ɩka 'lɔ wa tɩ, yɩ de wʋ nɩ a sɩ Soro yuor, na yɩ maal wʋ a lɛ na sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn puoro, na yɩ mɩ kʋ wʋ sʋ̃ʋfʋ jaa wʋn na bʋɔrɔ yi a yɩ sɛ̃. Bojũu wʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ sʋ̃ʋ nɩyɔɔ nɩ a maa mɩ̃ɛ.
45016003	Yɩ puor a Pɩrɩsɩla nɩ Akuila kʋ ma. Ba ɩ naa a n tʋ̃tʋ̃taaba a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ.
45016004	Ba tʋ̃n kũu tʋ̃mɔ̃ kʋ ma. A ba ɩ maa tɛɛ gba lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a pupuorbo bala ba jaa na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ɩ̃gãn mɩ 'maan ba naa.
45016005	Puor a pupuorbiir bala na ma lɔ̃ɔ puor a ba yir. Puor a n badaba Epainɩtʋsɩ, 'lɔ lɛ de nie turo a Kɩrɩsɩto be a Asɩya paal pɔ.
45016006	Yɩ puor a Mɛɛr mɩ na ir nyãa 'yɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ yɩ,
45016007	na yɩ mɩ puor a Andirunɩkasɩ nɩ a Junɩyasɩ. Ba ɩn a n bʋr nɩbɛ ka maa nɩ bala jaa mɩ dɔ̃ɔ 'mataa be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ. A nɩtʋ̃nsɩ bɔ̃ɔ ban jaa chɛchɛ, bala mɩ lɛ de nie turo a Kɩrɩsɩto tɩchɛ ka a maa wa bɩɛr.
45016008	Yɩ puor Ampɩlatusɩ kʋ ma, n nʋ̃ wʋ naa a Kɩrɩsɩto tufʋ jũu,
45016009	na yɩ mɩ puor Urbanusɩ na pʋɔ sɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ nɩ a n badaba Sɩtachɩsɩ.
45016010	Yɩ puor Apelesɩ nɩrɛ jaa na sɔɔ ɩka wʋ turo naa a Kɩrɩsɩto sɔr jaa nɛ nɛ nɛ, na yɩ mɩ puor Aristobulus nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa.
45016011	Yɩ puor a Hɛrɔdiyɔn na ɩ a n bʋr nɩrɛ, na yɩ mɩ puor a Narsɩsusɩ nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa na turo a sɩ Soro.
45016012	Yɩ puor a Tɩrafaina nɩ Tɩrafosa, a pɔbɔ ba nyãna mʋ̃ɔn nɩbir nɩ a sɩ Soro tʋ̃mɔ̃, na yɩ puor a Persis mɩ na ɩ a pɔɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ na mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a sɩ Soro tʋ̃mɔ̃.
45016013	Yɩ puor a Worofʋs ban ir a sɩ Soro pɔ nɩ a wʋ ma, a wʋ ma mɩ ɩn a n ma.
45016014	Yɩ puor Asɩnkirtusɩ, nɩ Filegon, nɩ Hɛmɩsɩ nɩ Patrobas nɩ Hermasɩ nɩ a yɛɛr bala jaa na be a ba sɛ̃.
45016015	Yɩ puor a Filologusɩ nɩ Juliya nɩ Nereyus nɩ a wʋ yɛpɔɔ nɩ Olinpasɩ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo ba jaa na be a ba sɛ̃.
45016016	Yɩ puor puor taa nɩ pʋpɛl. A pupuorbiir ba jaa puor yɩ naa nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto yuor.
45016017	N kpãkpãana yɩ naa yɛɛr ɩka yɩ guro yɩ mɩ̃ɛ sʋ̃ nɩ a bala na ma waara nɩ a ootaa, na ba ma vɛ̃ ka yɩ bãra loro a wiilfʋ nyã yɩn jãn pɔ. Yɩ tɔɔ 'laa tɩ bar ba.
45016018	Bojũu a nɩbɛ ba nyãna a ba ɩ a sɩ Soro Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala mɩ̃ɛ vɔlaa bomo lɛ ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ bʋɔrɔ. Ba ma 'yɛrɛ na jaa hɛ lɛ lɛ lɛ na ba de nɛnʋ̃ɔ bɛl a nɩbɛ bala tɩɛr na ba chen niem ɛ.
45016019	Nɩrɛ jaa wõn a lɛ yɩn turo a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nɛ nɛ nɛ, ka nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ sɩ a yɩ yele jũu. Tɩchɛ n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ maala vɩla nɩ yɛ̃, na yɩ ta bɔ̃ɔ yelbier maalfʋ ɛ.
45016020	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ a nyã'maar sʋɔ, a kʋ̃ lɛ kor ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a wʋ ŋmɩ̃ɛ a Satan a yɩ gbɛɛ pĩlem. A wɩ̃ɛfʋ na yi a sɩ Soro Yesu sɛ̃ a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
45016021	Timoti na ɩ a n tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ sʋɔ puor yɩ naa, ka a Lusiyusɩ nɩ Jason nɩ Sosipater na ɩ a n bʋr nɩbɛ mɩ puoro yɩ naa.
45016022	Maa mɩ na ɩ Tɛrtɩyɔsɩ na sɛɛrɛ a Pɔɔl gãn nyã mɩ puoro yɩ naa nɩ a sɩ Soro yuor.
45016023	Gayus yir maa nɩ pupuorbiir na kpɩɛrɛ a wʋ kaara sɩ mɩ puoro yɩ naa. Erastus na ɩ a tẽe libikaara nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a sɩ yɛbɛ Kuwartusɩ mɩ puoro yɩ naa.
45016025	Pʋ̃pãanyã, tɩɩr wʋ ta a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na sʋ̃ʋ yɩ a yɩ tʋ̃ɔ ara tu a n 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã ɩn mʋɔl na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto, naa chaar a yelsɔɔlaa nyãna na sɔɔl a kõr jaa na po.
45016026	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, a yelsɔɔlaa chaar naa tu a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn vʋr nyã na 'yɛr ba, ka a paalsɩ ba jaa na sɔɔ de, na ba turo wʋ.
45016027	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã tɛɛ lɛ ɩ a yɛ̃ sʋɔ, wʋ nyɛrɛ tɩɩr bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ. A ɩ a lɛ.
46001001	Maa Pɔɔl a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl a wʋ bɔfʋ pɔ ɩka n ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nãa nɩ a sɩ yɛbɛ Sosetenesɩ,
46001002	lɛ sɛɛrɛ a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a yɩn na puoro a Nãaŋmɩn be a Korɩntɩ tẽe pɔ. A yɩn na oo be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ na yɩ ɩ a wʋ nɩ chɛchɛsɩ lɔ̃ɔn a bala na be jie jaa na bʋɔlɔ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor na ɩ a sɩn nɩ a ba jaa Soro.
46001003	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃ a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
46001004	N ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan kʋ yɩ bojũu wʋ wɩ̃ɛ yɩ naa tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
46001005	A wʋ jũu lɛ yɩ le yele a jaa pɔ, a yɩ 'yɛrbie nɩ a yɩ bɔ̃ɔfʋ a jaa pɔ,
46001006	bojũu a Kɩrɩsɩto dãasɩɛ sɩn di, yɩ sɔɔn de.
46001007	A lɛ jũu, yaa faa a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kʋfʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ɛ, na yɩ pãa mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir chɛlɛ a lɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na lɛ lɩɛb wa.
46001008	Wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩn ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn tɩ tãn a baaraa, ka yɩ kʋ̃ tara chɛfʋ ɛ, tɩ tãn a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto waa bɩbir.
46001009	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã na bʋɔl yɩ wa lɔ̃ɔn a wʋ Bie Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ Soro ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ.
46001010	N yɛɛr, n den a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor naa sʋɔrɔ nɩ yɩ ɩka yɩ jaa yɩ ta ŋma dẽdẽ ka ootaa be a yɩ pɔ ɛ, a lɛ na vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ pãa tara nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩ tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen.
46001011	N yɛɛr, nɩbɛ bamɩne na yi a Kɩloe yir wa man kʋ ma ɩka nɛchɩrɛ ben a yɩ chara pɔ.
46001012	A lɛ par lɛ ɩka, a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ma 'yɛr ɩka, Pɔɔl lɛ maa turo, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr, Apolosɩ lɛ maa turo, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr, Sɩfasɩ lɛ n turo, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr ɩka, Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ n turo.
46001013	A Kɩrɩsɩto ŋman dẽdẽme bɩɩ? Pɔɔl lɛ ba kpa a daa ju bɩɩ? Bɩɩ Pɔɔl yuor lɛ yɩ son a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ?
46001014	N pʋɔ pɛl naa ɩn ba so a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ɛ, ka ala ba ɩ Kɩrɩsɩpusɩ nɩ Gayus tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ,
46001015	ka nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩka maa yuor lɛ n son yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
46001016	Ɔ̃ɔ, n mɩ dɔ̃ɔ so a Sɩtɛfanas nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ba jaa a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ. A anyã puor n ba tɩɛr nɩrɛ jaa ɩn lɛ so a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
46001017	Bojũu Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ba tʋ̃ ma ɩka n tɩ suoro nɩbɛ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ n tɩ mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ na ba ɩ nɩsaal yɛ̃ 'yɛr ɛ. Ka a Kɩrɩsɩto kũu wʋn kpi a daa taa ɩ pɔrɔ ɛ.
46001018	Bojũu a daa 'yɛr ɩn dãbol 'yɛr kʋ a bala na wɛrɛ, tɩchɛ a ɩn Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ a sɩn bala na nyɛ a faafʋ.
46001019	Bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Ɩn sɔ̃ɔ naa a yɛ̃ dẽme yɛ̃ bar, naa bʋ̃bʋr a bɔ̃ɔfʋ dẽme bɔ̃ɔfʋ bar."
46001020	Nyɩnɛ lɛ a yɛ̃ dẽme be? Nyɩnɛ lɛ a bɔ̃ɔfʋ sʋɔ be? Nyɩnɛ lɛ chɩbɛ dẽme mɩ be a dɩna? A ba ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɩɛb a wɛr nyã yɛ̃ a wʋ ɩ jɔl ɛ?
46001021	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn yɛ̃ kʋ vɛ̃ ka a wɛr de a wʋ yɛ̃ bɔ̃ɔn wʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ pɛl naa nɩ a jɔl mʋɔl ban mʋɔl ka a na faa a bala na sɔɔ de.
46001022	A Juu nɩbɛ ma bʋɔrɔ naa nɛ'maa yele, ka a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, mɩ bʋɔrɔ yɛ̃.
46001023	Tɩchɛ sɩn mʋɔl naa Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ban kpa a daa ju, ka a ɩ gbɛr bãrfʋ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ tɩ mɩ ɩ jɔl yele kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ.
46001024	Tɩchɛ a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na lɔ̃ɔ bʋɔl a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn yɛ̃.
46001025	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn jɔlʋ̃ ɩn yɛ̃ gar a nɩrɛ yɛ̃, ka a Nãaŋmɩn balfʋ tara kpɛ̃ɔ gar a nɩrɛ kpɛ̃ɔ.
46001026	N yɛɛr, yɩ tɩɛr a lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ be tɩ a Nãaŋmɩn wa bʋɔl yɩ, nɩsaal kaafʋ pɔ, a yɩ yɔɔ ba dɔ̃ɔ ɩ yɛ̃ dẽme ɛ, a yɩ yɔɔ ba dɔ̃ɔ ɩ yuor dẽme ɛ, yaa ɩ nãmɩne bibiir ɛ.
46001027	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn ir naa a wɛr nyã jɔl bon 'yɔ̃ɔn a yɛ̃ dẽme vɩ̃, Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ir naa a wɛr nyã bʋ̃balaa na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔn a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme vɩ̃.
46001028	Nãaŋmɩn ma ir naa a wɛr bon ba 'yɔ̃ɔnaa, a ala a nɩbɛ na kaara pɔrɔ, nɩ a nɩbɛ bala gba nɩrɛ jaa na ba 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ, wʋ ɩ naa nɩtɔ̃ ka a bon 'lɔ a wɛr na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ka wʋ ɩ pɔrɔ,
46001029	ka nɩrɛ jaa taa bʋɔrɔ yuor a wʋ niem ɛ.
46001030	A wʋ jũu lɛ yɩ be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a yɛ̃ yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ kʋ sɩ, na wʋ ɩ a sɩ torfʋ nɩ chɛchɛ nɩ a faafʋ.
46001031	A lɛ jũu, nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Vɛ̃ ka a 'lɔ na bʋɔrɔ yuor, wʋ bʋɔrɔ a yuor a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ."
46002001	N yɛɛr, ɩn dɔ̃ɔ wa a yɩ sɛ̃, n ba waan nɛbɔ̃ɔn bɩɩ yɛ̃ 'yɛr naa wa man a Nãaŋmɩn dãasɩɛ kʋ yɩ ɛ.
46002002	Bojũu a lɛ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ be a yɛ sɛ̃, n ba lɛ bɔ̃ɔ bon jaa pʋɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ban kpa a daa ju ɛ.
46002003	Balfʋ, dãbɩ̃ɛ nɩ mĩifʋ lɛ n dɔ̃ɔ ben a yɩ sɛ̃.
46002004	A n 'yɛr nɩ a n mʋɔlfʋ ba ɩ yɛ̃ 'yɛrbie ɛ, tɩchɛ a ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ wiilfʋ lɛ,
46002005	ka a yɩ sɔɔfʋ taa dɩɛl a nɩrɛ yɛ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ a dɩɛl a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ.
46002006	Faa nyɛ, sɩn ma 'yɛr a sɩ 'yɛr nɩ yɛ̃ kʋ a bala na nʋ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn sɔr pɔ, a ba ɩ a wɛr nyã bɩɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme yɛ̃ na wa ɩ pɔrɔ daar kɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
46002007	Kai, sɩn 'yɛrɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn yɛ̃ sɔɔlaa, a yɛ̃ 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔl a Nãaŋmɩn na kaa ir a sɩ daar kɔ̃ɔ tɩɩr jũu sɛrɛ na wʋ wa maal a wɛr.
46002008	A wɛr nyã kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme ba dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, ala ɩ bala ta bɔ̃ɔ ba kʋ̃ naa kpa a tɩɩr Soro a daa ju ɛ.
46002009	Tɩchɛ a lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Nɩbir jaa ba nyɛ ɛ, toor jaa ba wõ ɛ, tɩɛr jaa mɩ ba bɔ̃ɔn a ala a Nãaŋmɩn na chɔɔr kʋ a bala na nʋ̃ wʋ ɛ."
46002010	Tɩchɛ anyãna lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wiil kʋ sɩ, Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ma bɩɛr naa a yelsɩ a jaa, na wʋ gba ma bɔ̃ɔ a ala na be a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔm.
46002011	Nɩbuor lɛ bɔ̃ɔ lɛ na be a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ tɩɛr pɔ, ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ̃ɛ ba lɛ ɛ? A lɛ mɩ lɛ nɩrɛ ba bɔ̃ɔ lɛ na be a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɛr pɔ ɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ Sɩɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
46002012	A ba ɩ a wɛr nyã sɩɛ lɛ sɩ tara ɛ, tɩchɛ a Sɩɛ 'lɔ na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ a sɩ de bɔ̃ɔn a ala a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ sɩ a pɔrɔ.
46002013	A anyãna lɛ sɩ 'yɛrɛ, a ba ɩ nɩrɛ 'yɛrbie sɩn jãn ɛ, tɩchɛ 'yɛrbie ala sɩn jãn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛ̃ na sɩ wile nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a Sɩɛ 'yɛrbie.
46002014	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ba tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ɛ, maa sɔɔ a ala na yi a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛ̃ ɛ, bojũu a ɩn dãbol yele kʋ wʋ a wʋ maa bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, bojũu nɩrɛ na tʋ̃ɔn bɔ̃ɔ ala ɩ wʋ tara naa Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ.
46002015	A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ma vɩɛr naa a yele a jaa kaa, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ tɩɛr ɛ.
46002016	Bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "An lɛ bɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro tɩɛr, na wʋn kpãa wʋ?" Tɩchɛ sɩn lɛ tara a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tɩɛr.
46003001	N yɛɛr, n kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ nɩ yɩ fɩka nɩbɛ na tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ n 'yɛrɛ nɩ yɩ naa fɩka a wɛr nɩbɛ na yɩ ɩ bibiir a Kɩrɩsɩto sɔr pɔ.
46003002	Bɩrkʋ̃ɔ tɛɛ lɛ n kʋ yɩ a ba ɩ saa yɩn ba ta na tʋ̃ɔ di ɛ. Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ yɩ chɛnɛ ba ta ɛ.
46003003	Yɩ chɛnɛ na ɩrɛ fɩka nɩbɛ na ba bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, bojũu nyuur nɩ nɛchɩrɛ chɛnɛ na be a yɩ pɔ, yaa chɛnɛ ɩ a wɛr nɩbɛ ɛ? Na yɩ maala a lɛ ban maala ɛ?
46003004	A yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na ma 'yɛr, maa turo na Pɔɔl, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr ɩka, maa turo na Apolosɩ. Yaa chɛnɛ ɩrɛ fɩka nɩbɛ na ba bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ?
46003005	A anyãna a jaa pɔ, Pɔɔl nɩ a Apolosɩ, bo ba ɩ? Tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ lɛ sɩn ɩ a yɩ tu a be wa sɔɔ de ka a sɩ Soro kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa nɩ wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃.
46003006	Maa lɛ bʋr ka a Apolosɩ mɩ chɔr a kʋ̃ɔ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ so an nʋ̃ɔ.
46003007	Lɛ a 'lɔ na bʋr, nɩ a 'lɔ na chɔr a kʋ̃ɔ, ba ɩ bon jaa ɛ, tɩchɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ tɛɛ na vɛ̃ ka a bonsɩ a jaa nʋ̃ɔ.
46003008	A nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bʋr nɩ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na chɔr a kʋ̃ɔ ba jaa tara na tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na nyɛ a lɛ wʋn tʋ̃ sãyar.
46003009	Bojũu, sɩn ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃taaba, yɩn mɩ lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn puo, a Nãaŋmɩn yir wʋn mɩɛrɛ.
46003010	A wɩ̃ɛfʋ a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ ma lɛ so ka n kpar a dachin par kparaa nɩtãa bɔ̃ɔ mɩɛrɛ, ka a bamɩne mɩ mɩɛrɛ dɔɔlɔ. Tɩchɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ bɔ̃ɔ kaara a lɛ wʋn mɩɛrɛ dɔɔlɔ.
46003011	A yele lɛ ɩka, nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ kpar a dachin par kpar yuo lɛ pʋɔ a 'lɔ na be be ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto.
46003012	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ den sɛlma, kpãna, kʋsɩr kpɩ̃ɛn, daar, mʋɔr bɩɩ kakɩɛ,
46003013	nɩrɛ jaa na nyɛ naa a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃, bojũu a bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a jaa na gãn chãa pɔ. Bũu lɛ na vuul nɩrɛ jaa tʋ̃mɔ̃ na wʋ bɛɛr ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tʋ̃mɔ̃ kaa.
46003014	Ala ɩ a lɛ wʋn mɛ dɔɔl ba sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, wʋn nyɛn a wʋ sãyar.
46003015	Ala ɩ a wa di naa a nɩnyɩnɛ kʋ̃ nyɛ bon jaa ɛ, wʋn nyɛn faafʋ, tɩchɛ wʋn kaara naa fɩka nɩrɛ bũu na vuul.
46003016	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka yɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ka a wʋ Sɩɛ kpɩɛrɛ a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ?
46003017	Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa sɔ̃ɔ naa a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir nyã, Nãaŋmɩn na sɔ̃ɔ naa a nɩnyɩnɛ, bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir ɩn chɛchɛ. Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ a puorfʋ yir nyã.
46003018	Yɩ ta bɛlɛ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ tɩɛr naa ɩka wʋ ɩ naa yɛ̃ sʋɔ a wɛr nyã pɔ, wʋ lɩɛb ɩ "Jɔl" na wʋ pãa tʋ̃ɔ lɩɛb yɛ̃ sʋɔ.
46003019	Bojũu a wɛr nyã yɛ̃ ɩ naa jɔl yele a Nãaŋmɩn niem, nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ, "Wʋ ma nyɔɔ naa a yɛ̃ sʋɔ a wʋ yɛ̃ yele pɔ."
46003020	A lɛ sɛb go, "A Soro bɔ̃ɔ naa a yɛ̃ dẽme tɩɛr ka a ɩ pɔrɔ."
46003021	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ wʋ ta lɛ 'mɔɔrɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ nɩrɛ yele ɛ! Yɩn lɛ so a bonsɩ a jaa,
46003022	ka maa Pɔɔl lɛ bɩɩ, Apolosɩ lɛ bɩɩ, Sɩfasɩ lɛ bɩɩ, a wɛr lɛ bɩɩ, nyɛvʋr lɛ bɩɩ, kũu lɛ bɩɩ, dɩna lɛ bɩɩ, ka daar kɔ̃ɔ lɛ, yɩn lɛ so a jaa.
46003023	A Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ so yɩ, ka Nãaŋmɩn mɩ so a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto.
46004001	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ma kaa sɩ a sɩ ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na de a wʋ yelsɔɔlsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ nuur pɔ.
46004002	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a lɛ na gã lɛ ɩka a bala ban de bon 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba nuur pɔ, ba tara yelmɩ̃ɛ.
46004003	A ba bã ma ɛ, ala ɩ ka yɩn lɛ bɩɩ a wɛr nɩrɛ lɛ tɔɔrɔ a n 'yɛr sɩrɛ jaa a maa mɩ̃ɛ kʋ̃ tɔɔr a n 'yɛr ɛ.
46004004	N ba tɩɛr yele jaa ɩn ɩ bɔr ɛ, tɩchɛ a ba wiil ɩka n ba tara yele ɛ. A sɩ Soro lɛ na tɔɔr a n 'yɛr.
46004005	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta de nie tɔɔrɔ a 'yɛr ka a bɩbir ba ta ɛ. Yɩ chɛlɛ ka a sɩ Soro wa. 'Lɔ lɛ na yin yele a jaa na sɔɔl a libe pɔ, chãa pɔ, na wʋ mɩ wiil a ala na sɔɔl a nɩbɛ tɩɛr pɔ. A bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na nyɛ a wʋ pɛɛfʋ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
46004006	Pʋ̃pãanyã, n yɛɛr, a yɩn jũu lɛ n de a yele anyãna naa man a maa nɩ a Apolosɩ, ka yɩn jãn a par yi a sɩ sɛ̃ a lɛ ban 'yɛr ɩka, "Taa ɩrɛ wa chen po a lɛ ban sɛb ɛ." Ka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa pãa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩbɛ gara taa ɛ.
46004007	Ana lɛ maal yɩ a yɩ be yɩ yõ gar nɩrɛ jaa? Bo yɩ tara, ka a ba ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ yɩ ɛ? Ala ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ yɩ, ŋmɩnɛ a ɩ a yɩ bʋɔrɔ yuor fɩka yaa ɩ lɛ ɛ?
46004008	Yɩ ben tara bon jaa yɩn bʋɔrɔ! Na yɩ be ɩ taraa dẽme! Yɩ ben lɩɛb nãmɩne ka sɩn ba ɩ ɛ! Maa bɔfʋ lɛ fɩka yɩ ta ɩ a nãmɩne sɩrɛ jaa, ka a sɩ mɩ ta pʋɔ yɩ ɩ a nãmɩne.
46004009	Bojũu maa sɛ̃, a kaara naa fɩka a Nãaŋmɩn den a sɩn na ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ a sɩ pii a nɩyɔɔ puor, a ban kʋ sɩ chãa pɔ. Ka a sɩ ɩ bʋ̃manãa kʋ a wɛr nɩ a malakasɩ nɩ a nɩbɛ ba jaa.
46004010	Sɩn ɩn jɔlɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jũu tɩchɛ ka a yɩn ɩ yɛ̃n dẽme a wʋ pɔ. Sɩn ɩn nɩbaalsɩ tɩchɛ ka a yɩn ɩ kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme. Ba 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ yɩ naa tɩ kpɛrɛ sɩn.
46004011	Wa tãn dɩna gba, kɔ̃ nɩ kɔ̃nyũur lɛ sɩ ma chiine, ka a sɩ bʋ̃sursɩ chɩɛr chɩɛr ka ba pɔɔrɔ sɩ, saa tara yir kpɩɛrɛ ɛ.
46004012	Tʋ̃ kpɩ̃ɛn lɛ sɩ ma tʋ̃n a sɩ mɩ̃ɛ nuur, bala wa tʋ sɩ, sɩ ma 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ ba, bala sɔɔ gere sɩ, tɩ sɩ ma tara na kãnyir.
46004013	Bala wa sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a sɩ yuor, sɩ maa 'yɛr tuo ɛ, wa tãn dɩna, baa bʋɔlɔ sɩ bon jaa ɛ, ka a sɩ ɩ a wɛr wʋ jaa tãpuor ju sɔɔr.
46004014	N ba sɛɛrɛ a anyãna ɩka n su yɩ vɩ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka n kpãa yɩ maa mɩ̃ɛ bi'yɔ̃ɔnsɩ kaar.
46004015	Yɩn gba tara nɩbɛ turo pie (10,000) na kaara yɩ a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ, tɩ yaa tara sãamɩne yɔɔ ɛ, maa na wa mʋɔl a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ yɩ lɛ ɩ a yɩ sãa.
46004016	Ala lɛ so ka n pãa sʋɔrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩ turo a lɛ ɩn turo.
46004017	A anyãna jũu mɩ lɛ so ka n tʋ̃nɔ̃ a Timoti na ɩ a n bie ɩn nʋ̃, wʋ tara na yelmɩ̃ɛ a sɩ Soro pɔ. Wʋn tɩ jɛɔ yɩ naa a lɛ a n befʋ na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ, na n mɩ wile nɩ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ a jiir a jaa.
46004018	A yɩ bamɩne chɩɛrɛ nɩ nyãa ɩrɛ fɩka n kʋ̃ lɛ wa be go ɛ.
46004019	Tɩchɛ a kʋ̃ lɛ kor ɛ, ala ɩ a sɩ Soro sɔɔ naa, ɩn wan a yɩ sɛ̃, naa tɩ kaa a ba ɩ a bala na chɩɛrɛ a nyãa 'yɛrɛ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka n tɩ kaa a kpɛ̃ɔ buor ban tara.
46004020	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ yele ba ɩ nɛɛ 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ɩn kpɛ̃ɔ.
46004021	Buor sʋɔ lɛ yɩ bʋɔrɔ? Maa wa tɩrɛ, n tɩn kpaara bɩɩ nʋ̃fʋ nɩ jomm sɩɛ?
46005001	Ba wa man kʋ ma sɩrɛ jaa ɩka sɛ̃sɛ̃yele ben a yɩ pɔ, a lɛ gba na ba ɩrɛ a bala na ba puoro pɔ ɛ. Bie na na gãn a wʋ sãa pɔɔ.
46005002	Tɩ a yɩ chɛnɛ bʋɔrɔ yuor, vɩ̃ kʋ̃ naa nyɔɔ yɩ ka yɩ dii a nɩrɛ nyãna na maal a nɩtɔ̃ bar a yɩ pɔ ɛ?
46005003	A maa mɩ̃ɛ gba na ba be a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ a maa tɩɛr wʋ jaa ben a yɩ sɛ̃, naa gba tɔɔr a daba 'yɛr fɩka n ben be.
46005004	Yɩn wa lɔ̃ɔn a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor, a n tɩɛr mɩ ben a yɩ sɛ̃, ka a sɩ Soro Yesu kpɛ̃ɔ mɩ be be,
46005005	yɩ de a daba nyãna 'yɔ̃ɔ Satan nũu pɔ, ka wʋ sɔ̃ɔ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn bar, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn faa a wʋ sɩɛ a sɩ Soro bɩbir daar.
46005006	A yɩ yuor bɔfʋ nyã ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ. Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a dãbɩl jaa pʋʋr lɛ ma vɛ̃ ka a paanʋ̃ɔ vʋ̃ a yɔɔ ɛ?
46005007	Yɩ kpaar a dãbɩl koraa bar, tɩ na yɩ ɩ paanʋ̃ɔ paalaa na ba tara a dãbɩl ɛ. Lɛ lɛ yɩ kaara sɩrɛ jaa. Bojũu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ Gõl Bar Pɛɛraabile lon a sɩ bɔɔr.
46005008	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta ɩ a sɩ dire a Gõl Bar Difʋ nɩ a dãbɩl koraa ɛ, a dãbɩl koraa na ɩ yosɔ̃ɔ nɩ putuyele, tɩchɛ a ɩ a paanʋ̃ɔ na ba tara a dãbɩl ɛ. A paanʋ̃ɔ na ɩ chɛchɛ ɩfʋ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ tarfʋ.
46005009	A gãn 'lɔ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ sɛb kʋ yɩ, n 'yɛr ɩka yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ ɛ,
46005010	n ba 'yɛrɛ a bala na ba puoro na sɛ̃nɛ ɛ, bɩɩ a bɔgar dẽme, bɩɩ a nɩfɔlbɔ bɩɩ a tɩpuorbo ɛ. Ala ɩ lɛ lɛ, yɩ kʋ̃ naa yi a ka a wɛr nyã pɔ.
46005011	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, n sɛɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ, a lɛ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ ɩ nɩ nyã. Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa lɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a 'lɔ na bʋɔlɔ, a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a yɩ yɛbɛ tɩ na wʋ sɛ̃nɛ, nɩ bɔgar sʋɔ, na wʋ puoro tɩbɛ, nɩ yosɔ̃ɔnɔ̃, na wʋ ɩ dãburo, nɩ nɩfɔlɔ. A nɩrɛ nyãna tɔ sʋɔ, yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa 'mataa wʋ gba dire ɛ.
46005012	N tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ ɩka n tɔɔrɔ a bala na puoro 'yɛr, tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ yɩ kpãa a nɩbɛ bala yɩn 'mataa puoro nɩ na tʋ̃nɔ̃ a yelsɩ anyãna.
46005013	Nãaŋmɩn lɛ na tɔɔr a bala na ba puoro ɛ 'yɛr. "Yɩ dii a putusʋɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ bar a yɩ pɔ."
46006001	Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ wa nyɛn 'yɛr, ŋmɩnɛ a ɩ a wʋ na tara a 'yɛr chiin a 'yɛr tɔɔrbɔ bala na ba puoro ɛ jie, tɩ bar a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo jie?
46006002	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo lɛ na wa tɔɔr a bala na ba puoro 'yɛr ɛ? Ka ala ɩ yɩn lɛ na wa tɔɔr a bala na ba puoro 'yɛr, ŋmɩnɛ a yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ maal a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yelbil ɛ?
46006003	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka sɩn lɛ na tɔɔr a malakasɩ gba 'yɛr ɛ? Wa 'yɛrɛ nɩ a sɩ mɩ̃ɛ yelbil?
46006004	A lɛ jũu, yɩn wa tara a 'yɛrbil anyãna taaba, yɩ ma ir a pupuorbo bamɩne gba yɛ̃ na ba tal tɛɛr ɛ, ka ba tɔɔr a 'yɛr.
46006005	N 'yɛr naa anyãna na 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ vɩ̃, a ɩn sɩrɛ ɩka a yɩ pɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba tara yɛ̃ jaa pʋʋr na wʋn maal a wʋ taaba 'yɛr ɛ?
46006006	Tɩchɛ ka a yɛbɛ ma tara a yɛbɛ chiin a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie, a bala na ba ɩ a Yesu turbo sɛ̃.
46006007	Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ ɩka yɩ ben maal bɔr, bojũu yɩ ma nyɔɔr taa chiin a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie. Bo lɛ so ka yɩ kʋ̃ naa sɔɔ ka a nɩbɛ maal yɩ dɛɛr ɛ? Bɩɩ sɔɔ ka ba fɔl yɩ ɛ?
46006008	Tɩchɛ a yɩn mɩ̃ɛ fɔlɔ nɩ taa na yɩ maala taa dɛbɛ, na yɩ maala a anyãna kʋrɔ a yɩ yɛɛr.
46006009	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a putudẽme kʋ̃ kpɛ be a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ? Yɩ ta bɛlɛ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ, tɩpuorbo, a bala na fol bɩɩ a dɔɔr na lɩɛb gãna nɩ taa,
46006010	bɩɩ nãnyisɩ, bɩɩ a bɔgar dẽme, bɩɩ a dãburbo, bɩɩ a yosɔ̃ɔnbɔ, bɩɩ a nɩfɔlbɔ, ba ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa kʋ̃ kpɛ be a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ.
46006011	Lɛ lɛ a yɩ bamɩne mɩ dɔ̃ɔ kaara, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn pɛɛ yɩ bar, na wʋ oo yɩ ka yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ tu a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor nɩ a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pɔ.
46006012	A yɩ bamɩne 'yɛr naa ɩka, n ba chire bon jaa maalfʋ ɛ. Yele jaa ba chɩre maalfʋ ɛ. Tɩchɛ a ba ɩ yele a jaa lɛ vɩɛlɛ maalfʋ ɛ. Maa kʋ̃ sɔɔ ka bon jaa so ma ɛ.
46006013	Bamɩne mɩ ma lɛ 'yɛr naa ɩka, bʋ̃diir ben be puor 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a puor mɩ be be a bʋ̃diir 'yɔ̃ɔ. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn na sɔ̃ɔn a jaa ayi bar. Sɛ̃sɛ̃yele jũu ba lɛ a ɩ̃gãn be be ɛ, tɩchɛ a sɩ Soro jũu lɛ, ka a sɩ Soro mɩ be be a ɩ̃gãn jũu.
46006014	A kpɛ̃ɔ nyãna lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn sɩ̃ɩn a sɩ Soro a kũu pɔ, ka wʋ mɩ na sɩ̃ɩ sɩ a kũu pɔ.
46006015	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a yɩ ɩ̃gãma ɩn bʋ̃'yen nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto ɩ̃gãn ɛ? N pãa de a n ɩ̃gãn na ɩ bʋ̃'yen nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto ɩ̃gãn naa tɩ 'mar pɔɔ baa pɔ? N kʋ̃ ɩ a lɛ ɛ.
46006016	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka nɩrɛ 'lɔ na de a wʋ ɩ̃gãn tɩ 'mar a pɔɔ baa pɔ, ɩn bʋ̃'yen nɩ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn ɛ? Bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Ka ba jaa ayi ɩ ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen."
46006017	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na de wʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'mar a sɩ Soro, 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ ɩn bʋ̃'yen.
46006018	Yɩ tɔɔ yi a sɛ̃sɛ̃yele pɔ. Yelbier jaa nɩrɛ na ɩrɛ ma ben a wʋ ɩ̃gãn yõo, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na sɛ̃nɛ, a wʋ ɩ̃gãn lɛ wʋ maala a yelbier 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
46006019	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a yɩ ɩ̃gãn ɩn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ puorfʋ yir ɛ? A 'lɔ na be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ. A 'lɔ yɩn nyɛ yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɔ? Yaa so yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
46006020	Nãaŋmɩn da yɩn so. A lɛ jũu, yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a yɩ ɩ̃gãma.
46007001	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a yele ala yɩn sɛb kʋ ma, an taa vɩɛlɛ na ka daba ta kul pɔɔ ɛ.
46007002	Tɩchɛ an ɩ a sɛ̃sɛ̃yele na be be jũu, daba jaa wʋ kul a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ pɔɔ, ka a pɔɔ jaa mɩ kul a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ sɩrɛ.
46007003	Ka a sɩrɛ nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ pɔɔ na ma lɔ̃ɔ sɔ̃ɔ, lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a pɔɔ nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ sɩrɛ mɩ ma lɔ̃ɔ a sɔ̃ɔ.
46007004	A pɔɔ tɛɛ ba lɛ so a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɩ̃gãn ɛ, tɩchɛ a wʋ sɩrɛ lɛ so. A lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, a daba tɛɛ mɩ ba so a wʋ ɩ̃gãn ɛ, tɩchɛ a wʋ pɔɔ lɛ so.
46007005	Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa mɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa a gaa jie ɛ, ka ala ba wa ɩ yɩ man taa na yɩ kʋ taa sɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jũu ɛ. Ka yɩn wa sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn baar, a yɩ lɛ lɔ̃ɔ taa go, ka a Satan taa nyɛ yɩn kʋ̃ lɛ wa tʋɔrɔ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔrɔ bɛl yɩ ɛ.
46007006	N 'yɛr naa ɩka anyã tara na sɔr, a ba ɩ binfʋ lɛ ɛ.
46007007	N naa bʋɔrɔ naa fɩka a dɔɔr ba ta be a n kaar. Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tara na a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ wʋ, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa bon ma tɛɛ naa a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ bon.
46007008	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a yɩn bala na ba kul taa ɛ, nɩ a pɔɔkɔɛ, a vɩɛlɛ naa ba taa kulo taa ɛ, na ba jɩ̃nɛ nɩtãa lɛ ɩn jɩ̃nɛ.
46007009	Tɩchɛ bala ba wa tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ nyɔɔrɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, ba kul taa. Ala ɩ ba kul taa, a sãn ban jɛ̃ ka a vɔlaa kʋrɔ ba.
46007010	A bala na kul taa, a nɛbinãa lɛ a nyã, a ba ɩ maa lɛ 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ a sɩ Soro lɛ 'yɛr. A pɔɔ wʋ taa ɩrɛ wa bara a wʋ sɩrɛ ɛ.
46007011	Tɩchɛ 'lɔ wa bar a wʋ sɩrɛ, wʋ taa lɛ kulo daba go ɛ, bɩɩ wʋ lɩɛb tɩ 'maal a wʋ sɩrɛ. Daba mɩ wʋ taa dire a wʋ pɔɔ bara ɛ.
46007012	A anyã 'lɔ, maa lɛ 'yɛrɛ, a ba ɩ a sɩ Soro lɛ ɛ. Ala ɩ a Yesu turo ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔɔ ba ɩ a Yesu turo ɛ, tɩ sɔɔ ɩka wʋn jɛ̃n wʋ naa wʋ taa ɩrɛ wa dire wʋ bara ɛ.
46007013	Ala ɩ a pɔɔ mɩ lɛ ɩ a Yesu turo, tɩchɛ ka a wʋ sɩrɛ ba ɩ a Yesu turo ɛ, tɩ mɩ sɔɔ ɩka wʋn jɛ̃n wʋ naa, a pɔɔ nyɩnɛ mɩ wʋ taa bara a sɩrɛ ɛ.
46007014	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn kãan a danyɩnɛ na ba ɩ a Yesu turo ɛ, ka wʋ ɩ nɩsʋ̃ a wʋ pɔɔ na ɩ a Yesu turo jũu, ka a pɔɔ mɩ na ba ɩ a Yesu turo ɛ, mɩ ɩ nɩsʋ̃ a sɩrɛ na ɩ a Yesu turo jũu. Ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, a ba bibiir na ɩn bidɛbɛ, tɩchɛ a lɛ jũu ba ɩn bisʋ̃n.
46007015	Tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na ba ɩ a Yesu turo ɛ, 'lɔ wa chiine wʋ chiine. Fʋn ɩ a Yesu turo, ka daba lɛ, bɩɩ pɔɔ lɛ, ta ŋmaa wʋ sɔr ɛ. Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl sɩ naa ka sɩ kpɩɛrɛ nɩ nyã'maar.
46007016	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a ɩ a fʋ̃ʋ pɔɔ, ba bɔ̃ɔ ɩka fʋn tʋ̃ɔ faa a fʋ sɩrɛ ɛ? Bɩɩ a daba, faa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka fʋ mɩn tʋ̃ɔ faa a fʋ pɔɔ ɛ?
46007017	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ mɔ̃ be a jie 'lɔ a sɩ Soro na bin wʋ, nɩ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl wʋ. A binfʋ nyãna lɛ n bin kʋ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ ba jaa.
46007018	Nɩrɛ ŋmaan yʋɔr tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn wa bʋɔl wʋ bɩɩ? Wʋ taa ɩrɛ wa sɔɔlɔ a wʋ yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ ɛ. Nɩrɛ mɩ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl, ba ŋmaa a wʋ yʋɔr bɩɩ? Wʋ taa lɛ ŋmaara go ɛ.
46007019	Yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ ɩn pɔrɔ, ka a yʋɔr ba ŋmaafʋ mɩ ɩ pɔrɔ, Nãaŋmɩn yelbinsɩ fʋn turo lɛ ɩ yelkpɛ̃ɛ.
46007020	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ chɛnɛ a lɛ nɛ wʋn be tɩ a Nãaŋmɩn wa bʋɔl wʋ.
46007021	Gbãgbaar lɛ yɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl yɩ bɩɩ? Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a ɩ tuo kʋ yɩ ɛ, ala ɩ yɩ tara na sɔr na so yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, yɩn tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a lɛ.
46007022	Bojũu ala ɩ nɩrɛ ɩn gbãgbaa tɩchɛ ka a sɩ Soro wa bʋɔl wʋ, a nɩnyɩnɛ son wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a sɩ Soro jũu. Lɛ mɩ lɛ, nɩrɛ na so wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩchɛ ka a sɩ Soro wa bʋɔl wʋ, a nɩnyɩnɛ mɩ ɩ naa Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto gbãgbaa.
46007023	Nãaŋmɩn da yɩn da tuo, yɩ ta ɩ nɩrɛ jaa gbãgbaa ɛ.
46007024	Yɛɛr, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ben Nãaŋmɩn niem, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ chɛnɛ a lɛ nɛ wʋn be tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn wa bʋɔl wʋ.
46007025	Pʋ̃pãanyã a bala na ba kul taa sɛrɛ ɛ, n ba tara yele jaa a sɩ Soro na kʋ ma ɩka n 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ n tara na 'yɛr ɩn na 'yɛr an ɩ a sɩ Soro nɩbaal jũu, n sɔɔ naa ɩka n ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ ka yɩn sɔɔ de.
46007026	A dɩna yelwõnsɩ jũu, n tɩɛraa ɩka a ɩn vɩla ka nɩrɛ jaa kpɩɛrɛ wʋ yõ.
46007027	Fʋ kul pɔɔ bɩɩ? Taa ɩrɛ wa dire wʋ bara ɛ. Dakʋɔr lɛ fʋ ɩ bɩɩ, pɔɔ kʋɔr lɛ fʋ ɩ? Taa tɩɛrɛ pɔɔ bɩɩ sɩrɛ kulfʋ ɛ.
46007028	Tɩchɛ ala wa ɩ fʋ kul pɔɔ, faa maal yelbier ɛ, ka ala ɩ pɔɔsaraa mɩ kul sɩrɛ, waa maal yelbier ɛ. Tɩchɛ a bala na kul taa na kpɛ̃n yelwõnsɩ pɔ ka n kʋ̃ sɔɔl yɩ a yele nyãna ɛ.
46007029	Yɛɛr, bon ɩn 'yɛrɛ lɛ ɩka, a sɔ̃ɔ ɩn jaa ŋmaa. An yi a dɩna chiine, bala na tara pɔbɔ, ba maala fɩka baa tara pɔbɔ ɛ.
46007030	Bala na kõnõ, ba maala fɩka baa kõnõ ɛ, bala mɩ pʋɔ na pɛl, ba mɩ maala fɩka ba pʋɔ ba pɛl ɛ. Ka bala mɩ na da bon, ba maala fɩka a ba ɩ bala lɛ so bin ɛ.
46007031	Bala mɩ na tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a wɛr nyã bonsɩ, ba ta de ba mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a ala pɔ ɛ, bojũu a wɛr nɩ a wʋ bonsɩ a jaa poro na chiine.
46007032	Maa bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka yɩ ta tara yele jaa tɩɛr ɛ. An ɩ daba baa tara pɔɔ ɛ, a sɩ Soro yele lɛ wʋ ma tɩɛrɛ, lɛ wʋn na ɩ pɛl a sɩ Soro pʋɔ.
46007033	Tɩchɛ daba na tara pɔɔ a wɛr nyã yelsɩ lɛ wʋ ma tɩɛrɛ, lɛ wʋn na ɩ pɛl a pɔɔ pʋɔ.
46007034	Ka a wʋ tɩɛr maa gã jibʋ̃'yen ɛ. Ka a pɔɔ mɩ na ba kul sɩrɛ ɛ, bɩɩ pɔɔsarbile ma tɩɛrɛ a sɩ Soro yele. A wʋ bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka wʋ de a wʋ ɩ̃gãn nɩ a wʋ sɩɛ kʋ a sɩ Soro. Tɩchɛ pɔɔ na tara sɩrɛ, a wɛr nyã bonsɩ tɩɛr lɛ wʋ ma tara, lɛ wʋn na pɛl a wʋ sɩrɛ pʋɔ.
46007035	Yɩ mɩ̃ɛ sʋ̃ʋfʋ jũu lɛ n 'yɛrɛ nɩ a anyãna, a ba ɩ yele lɛ n bine kʋrɔ yɩ ɛ. N bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ kpɩɛrɛ a lɛ na tor na yɩ tara tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen kʋ a sɩ Soro.
46007036	Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa tɩɛr ɩka waa maal a lɛ na sɛɛ nɩ a pɔɔsarbile wʋn ŋmaan a bara ɛ, ka a pɔɔbile mɩ jɛ̃ kor, ka a sɛɛ ɩka ba kul taa, wʋ ɩ a lɛ wʋn tɩɛr, a ba ɩ bier ɛ. Ba kul taa.
46007037	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ tɩɛr na ba vavire ɛ, a wʋ tɩɛr ba fɩrɛ wʋ ka wʋ tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ a tɩɛr nyɔɔrɔ na wʋ 'yɛr a wʋ tɩɛr pɔ ɩka wʋ kʋ̃ kul a pɔɔsarbile ɛ, a nɩrɛ nyã mɩ maal a lɛ na tor.
46007038	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na kul a pɔɔsarbile wʋ maal vɩla, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na ba kul ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ maal vɩla gar.
46007039	Pɔɔ wa kul sɩrɛ, 'lɔ nɩ a sɩrɛ ben taa, tɩchɛ a sɩrɛ wa kpi wʋ tara na sɔr ɩka wʋ kul daba 'lɔ jaa wʋn bʋɔrɔ, tɩchɛ a danyɩnɛ wʋ ɩ Yesu turo.
46007040	Lɛ ɩn nyɛ lɛ ɩka, ala ɩ waa kul sɩrɛ ɛ, tɩ na wʋ jɩ̃nɛ, wʋn ɩn bɔɔsʋ̃n sʋɔ. N tɩɛr ɩka n mɩ tara na a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ.
46008001	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a bomo ala ban ma lon bɔɔr kʋ a tɩbɛ 'yɛr lɛ n bʋɔrɔ ɩka n 'yɛr. Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka sɩ jaa tara na bɔ̃ɔfʋ, ka a bɔ̃ɔfʋ ma wile wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, tɩchɛ nʋ̃fʋ ma vɛ̃n ka sɩ baa.
46008002	Nɩrɛ na tɩɛr ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔn bon kɔ̃ɔ, waa bɔ̃ɔ bon jaa sɛrɛ ɛ, a lɛ wʋn tɩɛr ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔ naa ɛ.
46008003	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nʋ̃ Nãaŋmɩn, Nãaŋmɩn bɔ̃ɔn naa nɩnyɩnɛ.
46008004	A bomo ala ban lon a tɩbɛ bɔɔr nʋ̃nɔ̃ 'wɔfʋ yele. Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a tɩɩ ba ɩ bon jaa a ka a wɛr pɔ ɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn ba lɛ be be go ɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen nyã tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
46008005	Ka ba gba bʋɔlɔ ŋmɩnsɩ, ka saaju lɛ, bɩɩ a ka a tẽe lɛ, sɩrɛ jaa lɛ ɩka ŋmɩn yɔɔ ben be, nɩ sorbo yɔɔ.
46008006	Tɩchɛ sɩn sɛ̃ 'lɔ, Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen, na ɩ a Sãa bʋ̃'yen, 'lɔ sɛ̃ lɛ a bonsɩ a jaa yi, 'lɔ jũu lɛ sɩ be be, Soro bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto, a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ bonsɩ a jaa tu wa, ka sɩ mɩ be be a wʋ jũu.
46008007	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ jaa ba lɛ bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna ɛ. Nɩbɛ bamɩne chɛnɛ na mɩlʋ̃ nɩ a tɩbɛ, bala wa ɔɔrɔ nʋ̃n jaa, ba ma tɩɛr ɩka tɩɩ nʋ̃n lɛ, ka a ba tɩɛr na bal a lɛ jũu, ba ma sɔ̃ɔ naa.
46008008	Tɩchɛ bʋ̃diir kʋ̃ vɛ̃ ka sɩ gbʋr Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, sɩn di yele jaa ba ɩrɛ sɩ ɛ. Sɩn mɩ baa di ɛ, yele jaa ba ɩrɛ sɩ mɩ ɛ.
46008009	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃ ka a lɛ yɩn maala nɩ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ sofʋ taa lɩɛb kʋsɩr bãraa kʋ a bala na ba kpɛ̃mɛ a ba sɔɔfʋ pɔ ɛ.
46008010	Ala wa ɩ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na ba kpɛ̃mɛ a wʋ sɔɔfʋ pɔ ɛ, wa nyɛ naa a fʋ̃ʋ na tara a bɔ̃ɔfʋ nyãna a fʋ tɩ dire a tɩɩ yir, a mɩ kʋ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ ka wʋ tɩ dire a ala ban lon a bɔɔr kʋ a tɩbɛ ɛ?
46008011	Ka a fʋ yɛbɛ nyã a wʋ sɔɔfʋ na ba kpɛ̃mɛ ɛ, 'lɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto na kpi kʋ, fʋ sɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa nɩ a fʋ bɔ̃ɔfʋ nyã bar.
46008012	Fʋ̃ʋ wa maal a bier nyã tɔ kʋ a fʋ yɛɛr, fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔn a ba tɩɛrsɩ baal, Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ̃ɛ lɛ fʋ maal a bier a lɛ nɛ.
46008013	A lɛ jũu, ala ɩ bon ɩn na di na vɛ̃n ka a n yɛbɛ lo yelbier pɔ, n kʋ̃ lɛ 'wɔb nʋ̃n jaa ɛ, na n taa wa vɛ̃ ka wʋ lo ɛ.
46009001	N ba so n mɩ̃ɛ bɩɩ? N ba ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nãa ɩ̃sʋɔ bɩɩ? N mɩ ba nyɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu nɩ nɩbir bɩɩ? A ba ɩ yɩn lɛ ɩ a sɩ Soro tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɩn tʋ̃, tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ?
46009002	Ala ɩ gba, n ba ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nãa bamɩne sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩ yɩn sɛ̃ 'lɔ, sɩrɛ jaa n ɩ naa! Bojũu yɩn lɛ ɩ a jɩ̃nɛ wiil sɩrɛ jaa ɩka n ɩ naa a nɩtʋ̃nãa a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ.
46009003	A anyãna lɛ na ɩ a maa 'yɛr ɩn na 'yɛr kʋ a bala na wa bɛrɛ ma a nɛɛ.
