48004023	A bie 'lɔ na ɩ a gbãgbaa pɔɔ bie, ba dɔɔ wʋn tu a lɛ nɩsaal na guor, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ mɩ na ɩ a sumɩne bie, ba dɔɔ wʋn tun a Nãaŋmɩn nɛtɩraa pɔ.
48004024	Sɩn tʋ̃ɔ de a pɔbɔ banyãna ayi man nɛtɩrsɩ ayi. Haga lɛ dɔɔ a gbãgbaa bibiir. 'Lɔ lɛ ara kʋ a nɛtɩraa 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na maal a Sinai Tɔ̃ɔ ju.
48004025	Haga ara na kʋ a Sinai Tɔ̃ɔ na be a Arabɩya fɩka a dɩna Jerusalɛm, bojũu 'lɔ lɛ dɔɔ a wʋ bibiir ka ba ɩ a nɛbinãa gbãgbaar.
48004026	Tɩchɛ a Jerusalɛm 'lɔ na be a saaju son wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a sɩ ma.
48004027	Bojũu a sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Tara pʋpɛl, a fʋ̃ʋ pɔɔ abbaa, na ba dɔɔ bibiir ɛ. Yiele ŋmiere nɩ chɛlsɩ, fʋ̃ʋ nyã na ba wõ bie dɔɔfʋ tuo ɛ. A pɔɔ nyã na ba dɔ̃ɔ dɔɔ ɛ, bojũu a wʋ bibiir waan gar a pɔɔ 'lɔ na kul sɩrɛ."
48004028	Pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩn a n yɛɛr, yɩ kaara fɩka a Isaakɩ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛtɩraa bibiir.
48004029	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban dɔɔ a bie 'lɔ a ɩ̃gãn pɔ, wʋ ge naa a bie 'lɔ ban dɔɔn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ. Lɛ mɩ lɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã.
48004030	Tɩchɛ bo lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn 'yɛr? "Dii a gbãgbapɔɔ nɩ a wʋ bie bar, bojũu a bie 'lɔ na ɩ a gbãgbapɔɔ bie kʋ 'mataa din a Nãaŋmɩn nãbonsɩ nɩ a bie 'lɔ a sumɩne na dɔɔ ɛ."
48004031	A lɛ jũu n yɛɛr, saa ɩ a gbãgbaa pɔɔ bibiir ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩ ɩn a pɔɔ sumɩne bibiir.
48005001	A Kɩrɩsɩto faa sɩ naa, ala lɛ so ka sɩ so sɩ mɩ̃ɛ. A lɛ jũu, yɩ pãa ara kpɛ̃ɔ na yɩ ta lɛ de yɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ gbãgbaa tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ ɛ.
48005002	Yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a n 'yɛrbie jɩ̃nɛ. Maa Pɔɔl lɛ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka ala ɩ yɩ ŋman a yɩ yɔɩ, a Kɩrɩsɩto kʋ tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ yɩ ɛ.
48005003	N lɛ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa ɩka nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ŋmaa yʋɔr tara na sɔr ɩka wʋ sɔɔ a Juu nɩbɛ nɛbinsɩ a jaa.
48005004	A yɩn bala na bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ nyɛ faafʋ tu a nɛbinãa 'yɔ̃ɔ, ŋmaan yi a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, yɩ ŋmaan yi a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ pɔ.
48005005	Tɩchɛ a sɔɔfʋ jũu, sɩ chɩlɛ na nɩbijɩɛ ɩka sɩn nyɛn a Sɩɛ tɩɛrtɔ jie yeltorsɩ.
48005006	A Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka nɩrɛ ŋmaan yʋɔr bɩɩ ka waa ŋmaa yʋɔr ɛ, a ba wiil yele jaa ɛ. A yele 'lɔ na fɛr lɛ ɩka sɔɔfʋ na wile wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tun nʋ̃fʋ pɔ.
48005007	Yɩ dɔ̃ɔ joro jovɩla, an lɛ ŋmaa yɩ sɔr ɩka yɩ ta sɔɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ?
48005008	A sʋɔrfʋ nyã bʋrɔ ba yi a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bʋɔl yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ.
48005009	Fɩka dãbɩl bɩ̃lãa na ma vɛ̃ ka jɔ̃ vʋ̃, lɛ lɛ yele jaa pʋʋr bile ma sɔ̃ɔ yelyɔɔ.
48005010	N tara na sɔɔfʋ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ ɩka yɩ kʋ tɩɛr tɩɛr yuo ɛ. A nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na vɛ̃ ka a yɩ tɩɛr va vire na nyɛn gefʋ.
48005011	N yɛɛr, ba kʋ̃ ge ma ɛ, ala ɩ n 'yɛr yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ 'yɛr. A lɛ wiil ɩka a Yesu daa suur difʋ baar naa.
48005012	Ɩn naa bʋɔrɔ na ɩka a bala na ba vɛ̃ ka a yɩ tɩɛr gãna jibʋ̃'yen nɩ a ba yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ yele ɛ, ba ŋme a ba mɩ̃ɛ lãma.
48005013	Yɩn a n yɛɛr Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl ka yɩ so yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ta de a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ sofʋ nyãna maala nɩ yelbier ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ de a mɩ̃ɛ sofʋ nyã, na yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ taa nɩ nʋ̃fʋ.
48005014	A Nãaŋmɩn nɛbinsɩ a jaa, ba den sɛb 'yɛrbibʋ̃'yen tɛɛ, "Nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kaar."
48005015	Yɩn maa wa sɔɔ dʋ̃nɔ̃ taa na yɩ ɔɔrɔ taa, yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, na yɩ taa sɔ̃ɔ taar ɛ.
48005016	A lɛ jũu, n 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩ kpɩɛrɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na wile, na yɩ ta maala a lɛ a ɩ̃gãn na bʋɔr ɛ.
48005017	Bojũu bon 'lɔ a ɩ̃gãn na bʋɔrɔ ba ɩ a bon 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na bʋɔr ɛ. Bon 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ mɩ na bʋɔrɔ ba ɩ a bon 'lɔ a ɩ̃gãn mɩ na bʋɔr ɛ. A ma jɛɛrɛ nɩ taa na a na ŋmaa yɩ sɔr ka yɩ kʋ tʋ̃ɔ maal a lɛ yɩn bʋɔr ɛ.
48005018	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ben a yɩ pɔ, yaa lɛ chɛnɛ ɩ a nɛbinãa gbãgbaar ɛ.
48005019	A ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ ma gãn chãa pɔ, ala lɛ a anyãna sɛ̃fʋ, nɩ dɛɛr maalfʋ, nɩ jɔl dɩ̃ɛn,
48005020	nɩ tɩbɛ puorfʋ, nɩ sɔyele, nɩ 'laarfʋ, nɩ nɛchɩrɛ, nɩ nyuur, nɩ suur, nɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'mɔɔfʋ, nɩ ootaa,
48005021	nɩ nyuur, nɩ dãa buufʋ, nɩ dãnyugbulo, nɩ a ala na nyɛtãan a anyãna. N kpãana yɩ naa nɩtãa a lɛ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ de nie kpãa yɩ ɩka, a bala na maala a anyãna, kʋ̃ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ.
48005022	Tɩchɛ anyã lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wɔ̃mɔ̃, nɩ nʋ̃fʋ, nɩ chɩlfʋ, nɩ nyã'maar, nɩ kãnyir, nɩ nɩbaal kaafʋ, nɩ vɩla maalfʋ, nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ,
48005023	nɩ jomm ɩfʋ, nɩ mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔfʋ. Nɛɛ jaa ba be be gar a anyãna ɛ.
48005024	A bala na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ kpan a ba ɩ̃gãn nɩ a wʋ vɔlaa a daa ju.
48005025	Ala ɩ sɩn nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ lɛ 'mataa kpɩɛrɛ, yɩ vɛ̃ ka sɩn nɩ a 'lɔ 'mataa chiine.
48005026	Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka sɩ wile sɩ mɩ̃ɛ na sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa suur, tara taa nɩ nyuur ɛ.
48006001	N yɛɛr, ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ wa maal yelbier bɔr a sɔɔfʋ sɔr pɔ, fʋ̃ʋ nyã na tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ, tɔɔ wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɔr pɔ nɩ mɩ̃ɛ siirfʋ. Tɩchɛ gu a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ na fʋ mɩ taa lo a bɛɛr kaa pɔ ɛ.
48006002	Yɩ tuoro taa a yelwõnsɩ. Yɩn wa ɩrɛ a lɛ, yɩ turo naa a Kɩrɩsɩto nɛɛ.
48006003	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ wa tɩɛr ɩka wʋ ɩn bon kɔ̃ɔ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn ba ɩ bon jaa ɛ, wʋ mɩ̃ɛ lɛ wʋ bɛlɛ.
48006004	Nɩrɛ jaa wʋ ma bɛɛr a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tʋ̃mɔ̃ kaa tɩ na wʋ pãa chɩɛrɛ a nyãa na wʋ ta de a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ mana nɩ a wʋ taaba tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ.
48006005	Bojũu ɩ̃sʋɔ na ma tuon a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tuor.
48006006	A bala ban wiil, ba mɩ põ a ba bʋ̃tarsɩ kʋ a bala na wile ba.
48006007	Yɩ ta bɛlɛ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, nɩrɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ la Nãaŋmɩn ɛ. A bon 'lɔ fʋn bʋr, 'lɔ lɛ fʋn ŋma.
48006008	Fʋ̃ʋ nyã na bʋr a ala na ɩ a ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa, fʋn ŋman bʋ̃dɛbɛ. Ala ɩ fʋ bʋr a ala na pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pʋɔ, na tun a Sɩɛ pɔ ŋma nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
48006009	Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka sɩ bal nɩ vɩla maalfʋ ɛ, bojũu sɩn ŋma naa a ŋmafʋ sɔ̃ɔ, sɩn baa wa tɛɛ bar ɛ.
48006010	A lɛ jũu, sɩn wa nyɛ vuo, yɩ vɛ̃ a sɩ de maal vɩla kʋ nɩrɛ jaa, na sɩ mɔ̃ maal yɔɔ jaa kʋ a bala na be a sɔɔfʋ pɔ.
48006011	Maa wa sɛɛrɛ nɩ a maa mɩ̃ɛ nũu, nyɛ lɛ a sɛbie na ma ɩ a bɛrɛ jɩ̃.
48006012	A bala na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba wile a ba mɩ̃ɛ a ɩ̃gãn pɔ, bala lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba fɩr yɩ ka yɩ ŋma a yɔɩ. A yele 'lɔ yɔɔ ban ɩrɛ a lɛ, baa bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba nyɛ gefʋ a Kɩrɩsɩto daa jũu ɛ.
48006013	A bala gba mɩ na ŋma a yɔɩ ba turo a nɛbinãa ɛ, tɩchɛ ba bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩn yɩ ŋma a yɩ yɔɩ ka ba na chɩɛrɛ nyãa ɩka bala lɛ ŋma yɩ.
48006014	N taa ɩrɛ wa chɩɛrɛ nyãa bon jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ ka ala ba wa ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto daa ba lɛ ɛ. A lɛ jũu lɛ so, ka a wɛr nyã ju ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ ma ɛ, ka mɩ ba ɩ bon jaa kʋ a wɛr ɛ.
48006015	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ ŋmaan yʋɔr bɩɩ ka 'lɔ ba ŋmaa yʋɔr ɛ, a ba wiil yele jaa ɛ, tɩchɛ a lɛ na sɛɛ lɛ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ nyɛ dɔɔ paalaa.
48006016	A bala jaa na turo a sɔr nyãna, nyã'maar nɩ nɩbaal kaafʋ wʋ be a ba sɛ̃. Ba la lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kaa ir.
48006017	An yi a pʋ̃pãanyã chiine, nɩrɛ jaa wʋ ta lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ma yele go ɛ, bojũu a Yesu fɛlsɩ ben a n ɩ̃gãn pɔ.
48006018	N yɛɛr, ka a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ, a be a yɩ sɩɩr pɔ. A ɩ a lɛ.
49001001	Maa Pɔɔl a Nãaŋmɩn na sɔɔ ka n ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nãa lɛ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ a yɩn na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ be a Efesus na yɩ sɔɔ de a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto.
49001002	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃ a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
49001003	Pɛɛfʋ wʋ ta a Nãaŋmɩn, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto Sãa. Wʋn de a Sɩɛ yelsʋ̃n a jaa na be a saaju na wʋ sʋ̃ʋn sɩ, sɩn be a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ jũu.
49001004	Bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ ir sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ, tɩ na wʋ wa maal a wɛr ka sɩ na ɩ chɛchɛ na sɩ kʋ̃ tara chɛfʋ a wʋ niem ɛ, a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ jũu.
49001005	Nãaŋmɩn den nie ir sɩ ka sɩ ɩ a wʋ bibiir tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ. A ɩ naa a wʋ bɔfʋ naa pɛl a wʋ pʋɔ.
49001006	Ala lɛ so a sɩ pɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn maal vɩla kpɛ̃ɛ nyã wʋn maal sɩ na wʋ kʋ sɩ a wʋ Binʋ̃nãa.
49001007	A wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ sɩ nyɛ faafʋ tu a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ jũu. Sɩ nyɛn vɛ̃ kʋfʋ, an ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ bɛrma naa.
49001008	Wʋ maal sɩn vɩla tɩ põn bar, na wʋ kʋ sɩ par bɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ yɛ̃ a jaa.
49001009	An ɩ wʋ vɛ̃n ka sɩ bɔ̃ɔ a yelsɔɔlaa na be a wʋ tɩɛr pɔ, a ala wʋn bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ maal a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
49001010	Ka a ɩ sɩrɛ ɩka, wʋn kaal a bonsɩ a jaa na be a saaju nɩ ala na be ka a tẽe lɔ̃ɔ taa ka a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ bʋ̃'yen kaara ba, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto.
49001011	A wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ Nãaŋmɩn ir sɩ, wʋ kãan ir sɩ a lɛ na ɩ a wʋ pʋtɩɛr na wʋn maal yele a jaa ka a ɩ a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ.
49001012	A ɩ naa lɛ, ka a sɩn na ɩ a nɩdɔ̃ɔ na tara a Yesu a sɩ tɩɛrtɔ jie ka ban pɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn.
49001013	A yɩn mɩ dɔ̃ɔ pʋɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ yɩn wõ a yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ, a 'yɛr nyã na ɩ a yɩ faafʋ 'yɛr. Yɩn wa sɔɔ de wʋ, Nãaŋmɩn den a wʋ Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ 'yɔ̃ɔn yɩ jɩ̃nɛ.
49001014	A Sɩɛ nyã lɛ ɩ a tɛlma ɩka sɩn nyɛ naa ala Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ na wʋ faa a bala na ɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ a sɩ pɛɛrɛ wʋ.
49001015	A nyã jũu lɛ so, maa na wõ a yɩ yele a lɛ yɩn sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro Yesu nɩ a lɛ yɩn nʋ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ.
49001016	N ma dãna na Nãaŋmɩn a yɩ jũu, naa sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ yɩ.
49001017	Naa chɛnɛ sʋɔrɔ a tɩɩr Sãa, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na turo a wʋ nɛɛ ɩka wʋ kʋ yɩ a Sɩɛ yɛ̃, na wʋ wiil yɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yelwiilsɩ, ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ wʋ jaa chɛchɛ.
49001018	N sʋɔrɔ na Nãaŋmɩn ɩka wʋ chɩlʋ̃ a yɩ tɩɛr, ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a tɩɛrtɔ 'lɔ jũu wʋn bʋɔl yɩ, ka yɩ kʋ̃ tara baal ɛ, tɩ na yɩn tɩ de a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nãbomo wʋn tɩr nɛɛ kʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ.
49001019	A wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ na gar a jaa kʋ a sɩn na sɔɔ de wʋ, a kpɛ̃ɔ nyãna lɛ wʋ tʋ̃n a kpɛ̃ɔ tʋ̃mɔ̃.
49001020	'Lɔ lɛ wʋ de sɩ̃ɩn a Kɩrɩsɩto a kũu pɔ, na wʋ vɛ̃ ka wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ jie be a saaju.
49001021	Wʋ gar a tʋ̃ɔfʋ a jaa, nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, nɩ a sɩgãdaar ba jaa, nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ ba jaa, a ba ɩ a bala na be be a dɩna tɛɛ ɛ, tɩ a bala na wa be be daar kɔ̃ɔ.
49001022	Nãaŋmɩn den a bomo a jaa bin a wʋ gbɛɛ pĩlem, na wʋ ir wʋ ka wʋ ɩ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ ba jaa ju,
49001023	na ɩ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn, ka ba sɛɛn wʋ jaa, 'lɔ lɛ sɛɛ ba jaa, a jiir a jaa.
49002001	Yɩn 'lɔ, yɩ dɔ̃ɔ kpi be a yɩ maal dɛbɛ nɩ a yɩ yeldɛbɛ pɔ,
49002002	ala pɔ lɛ yɩ dɔ̃ɔ be, na yɩ turo a wɛr nyã sɔɩ nɩ a 'lɔ na di a sɛsɛbɛ nãa Satan. A sɩɛ nyã lɛ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a bawõnsɩ pɔ.
49002003	Sɩ jaa mɩ dɔ̃ɔ be a lɛ a ba kaar maala a lɛ a ɩ̃gãn na bʋɔrɔ, na sɩ turo a sɩ tɩɛr nɩ a ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa. Ka a Nãaŋmɩn suur mɩ dire nɩ sɩ a ba kaar.
49002004	Tɩchɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbaal na waa jũu, ka wʋ nʋ̃ sɩ yɔɔ jaa.
49002005	Wʋ maal sɩn ka sɩ 'mataa ir a Kɩrɩsɩto a kũu pɔ an ɩ sɩ dɔ̃ɔ kpi a yeldɛbɛ pɔ, a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ lɛ wʋ faan sɩ.
49002006	Nãaŋmɩn 'mantaa sɩ̃ɩn sɩ nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto ka sɩ 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ nɩ wʋ be a saaju.
49002007	A ɩ naa nɩtɔ̃ ɩka a ber ala na waara ka wʋ na wiil sɩ a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ na bɛr ma nɩ a wʋ maal vɩla a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
49002008	Bojũu a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ lɛ so yɩn nyɛ faafʋ tu a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ, a ba yi a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ sɛ̃ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ lɛ.
49002009	A ba ɩ yɩn tʋ̃mɔ̃ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ ka ɩ̃sʋɔ na chɛ nyãa ɛ.
49002010	Sɩ ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn nũu bʋ̃maalsɩ wʋn mɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka sɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃ tʋ̃sʋ̃n ala wʋn de nie chɔɔr bar ka sɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃.
49002011	A lɛ jũu, yɩ tɩɛr kaa a kõro a yɩn na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka a Juu nɩbɛ bʋɔlɔ yɩ a, yɔrwʋʋr dẽme, tɩ bʋɔlɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ a yɔrŋmaar dẽme, na ɩ a ɩ̃gãn nyã tɛɛ yele.
49002012	Yɩ tɩɛr kaa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩka yaa bɔ̃ɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto ɛ, ka yɩn yaa mɩ pʋɔ a Isɩral nɩbɛ pɔ ɛ, na yaa pʋɔ a nɛtɩrsɩ ala a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ kʋ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ. Yaa tara tɩɛrtɔ jie ɛ, na yaa lɛ bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ.
49002013	Yɩn bala na dɔ̃ɔ jãa tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩ wa gbʋr a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na yɩ be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ jũu.
49002014	Bojũu, a Yesu mɩ̃ɛ lɛ ɩ a sɩ nyã'maar, na wʋ maal a nɩbʋrsɩ ayi ka ba ɩ bʋ̃'yen, na wʋ ŋmɛr a dachin 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ var a sɩ ɩ a dɔ̃dẽme.
49002015	A Juu nɩbɛ nɛbinãa tara na chire yɔɔ, tɩchɛ Kɩrɩsɩto kũu sɔ̃ɔn a jaa. A wʋ bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka wʋ vɛ̃ ka a Juu nɩbɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɩ nɩpaalaa bʋ̃'yen, lɛ lɛ wʋ maal a nyã'maar.
49002016	Wʋ 'maal Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ba ka ba ɩ bʋ̃'yen. A kũu wʋn kpi a daa ju lɛ wʋ de kʋn a ba 'laar taa.
49002017	Wʋ wa mʋɔl naa a nyã'maar 'yɛr kʋ yɩn bala na jãa nɩ a bala na gbʋr.
49002018	Bojũu a tu naa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ka sɩ tara sɔr na ta a Sãa sɛ̃ nɩ a Sɩɛ bʋ̃'yen 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
49002019	A lɛ jũu, yaa lɛ chɛnɛ ɩ sãanba nɩ nɩyʋɔrsɩ go ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩn nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔn tẽe na yɩ ɩ a wʋ yir dẽme.
49002020	Ba mɩ mɛn dɔɔl a dachin par kparaa na ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ, ka a Yesu ɩ a sãlsɔɔ wɛɛ.
49002021	A wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a yir wʋ jaa choo taa na wʋ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir chɛchɛ 'lɔ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ.
49002022	Bojũu yɩ jaa ɩ naa a Kɩrɩsɩto tʋɔr, ka wʋ mɩ mɛ yɩ 'matãan a yir nyã pɔ, ka Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ kpɩɛrɛ.
49003001	Bon nɩ so ka n sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ yɩ lɛ ɩka, n ben pɔɔfʋ die pɔ bojũu ɩn mʋɔl a Yesu yele kʋ a yɩn na ba ɩ Juu nɩbɛ ɛ.
49003002	Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ yɩ wõ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋn kʋ ma a tʋ̃mɔ̃ nyãna a yɩ jũu.
49003003	A yelsɔɔlaa nyã lɛ wʋ wiil ma ka n bɔ̃ɔ naa de nie sɛb a ŋmaa kʋ yɩ.
49003004	Yɩn wa kar a ala, yɩn pãa bɔ̃ɔn naa a lɛ ɩn bɔ̃ɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto yelsɔɔlaa ala nɩrɛ na ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
49003005	Nãaŋmɩn ba dɔ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka a kõr dẽme bɔ̃ɔ a anyãna ɛ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã wʋ wiil kʋ a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nsɩ chɛchɛsɩ nɩ a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ chɛchɛsɩ tu a wʋ Sɩɛ pɔ.
49003006	A yelsɔɔlaa nɩ nyã ɩka a tu naa a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã pɔ, ka a yɩn na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, nɩ a Isɩral nɩbɛ na lɔ̃ɔn ŋmabʋ̃'yen, na ba 'mataa a ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen pɔ, ka ban 'mataa põ a nɛɛ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
49003007	N lɩɛb a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ tu a kʋfʋ nyã a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ na wʋ kʋ ma tu a wʋ tʋ̃kpɩ̃ɛn pɔ.
49003008	An ɩ maa lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ba jaa bɩr baaraa tɩchɛ ka a wɩ̃ɛfʋ nyã kʋ ma sɔr ɩka n mʋɔl a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, nɩrɛ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ ɛ,
49003009	ka n vɛ̃ ka a yelsɔɔlaa nyã chaar kʋ nɩrɛ jaa an ɩ a dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔl a kõr jaa a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ na maal a bonsɩ a jaa.
49003010	A wʋ bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka a pʋ̃pãanyã, wʋ tu a pupuorbiir pɔ wiil a wʋ yɛ̃ ka a tʋ̃ɔfʋ dẽme, nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme na be a saaju bɔ̃ɔn.
49003011	A anyãna lɛ wʋ tɩɛr a kõr jaa na wʋ wa de a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto a sɩ Soro na wʋ maal a wɛr.
49003012	Tu a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩn sɔɔ de wʋ jũu, sɔr gãn kʋ sɩ a sɩn 'la chen a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
49003013	A lɛ jũu n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka yɩ ɩ̃gãn sal ɩn dire dɔɔyɛ a yɩ jũu ɛ, a ɩ naa a yɩ tɩɩr yele lɛ.
49003014	A anyãna jũu lɛ n ma de gbur dumo a Sãa niem.
49003015	'Lɔ lɛ a balsɩ ba jaa Sãa, a bala na be a saaju nɩ a ba nyã na be ka a wɛr pɔ.
49003016	N sʋɔrɔ wʋ naa ɩka a yi a wʋ tɩɩr pɔ, ka wʋ de a wʋ Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔn yɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn, a yɩ kpɛ̃mɛ a ɩ̃gãn pʋɔm,
49003017	ka a Kɩrɩsɩto kpɩɛrɛ a yɩ nyãa pɔ, yɩn sɔɔ de wʋ jũu. A n sʋɔrfʋ lɛ ɩka, yɩ ba nyɩbɛ ara jaa chɩ̃chɩ̃ a nʋ̃fʋ pɔ,
49003018	a yɩn nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ na 'mataa nyɛ a lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto nʋ̃fʋ na yalʋ̃, nɩ a wʋ wõo, nɩ a dofʋ, nɩ a lɛ wʋn suu a pĩlem,
49003019	na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a nʋ̃fʋ na gar a bɔ̃ɔfʋsɩ a jaa, a yɩ pãa be a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na be.
49003020	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a 'lɔ na ma tʋ̃ɔ maal yele a jaa gar a lɛ sɩn sʋɔr wʋ, bɩɩ a lɛ sɩn tɩɛr nɩtãa lɛ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ na tʋ̃nɔ̃ a sɩ pɔ,
49003021	'lɔ lɛ so a tɩɩr a pupuorbiir pɔ, nɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
49004001	Ala lɛ so a maa ban pɔɔ a die pɔ a sɩ Soro jũu kpãkpãana yɩ ɩka, yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ kpɛfʋ vɩɛlɛ nyɛtãan lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl yɩ.
49004002	Yɩ siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ na yɩ bal yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, na yɩ tara kãnyir, na yɩ diere taa nɩ nʋ̃fʋ.
49004003	Yɩ mɔ̃ na yɩ vɛ̃ ka a Sɩɛ bʋ̃'yen ɩfʋ 'lɔ pɔ, a yɩ tara taa nɩ nyã'maar.
49004004	Bojũu ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen lɛ be be, nɩ a Sɩɛ bʋ̃'yen, nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl yɩ, ka yɩ tara tɩɛrtɔ jie bʋ̃'yen.
49004005	Soro bʋ̃'yen lɛ be be, sɔɔfʋ bʋ̃'yen nɩ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ bʋ̃'yen.
49004006	Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ, na wʋ ɩ a sɩ jaa Sãa, na wʋ kaara nɩrɛ jaa, na wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a ba jaa jie, na wʋ be a ba jaa pɔ.
49004007	Tɩchɛ a sɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa nyɛn a wɩ̃ɛfʋ kʋfʋ dẽdẽme nɩtãa lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na põ.
49004008	A anyãna lɛ so an sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ naa 'yɛr, "A lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ do, a wʋ sãma dẽme wʋn nyɔɔr turo wʋ naa, ka wʋ de bomo kʋ nɩbɛ."
49004009	A dofʋ par nɩ bo? Wʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ de nie suu a tẽe pɔ.
49004010	A 'lɔ na suu, 'lɔ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ do gar a saaju wʋ jaa, na wʋ sɛɛ a bonsɩ a jaa.
49004011	'Lɔ lɛ põ a nɩbɛ a tʋ̃mɔ̃, ka bamɩne ɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ, ka bamɩne ɩ a 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ, ka a bamɩne ɩ a 'yɛr mʋɔlbɔ, ka bamɩne mɩ kaara a nɩbɛ na ba wile ba.
49004012	Wʋ maal a nɩtɔ̃ ɩka wʋ chɔɔr a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ gun a tʋ̃mɔ̃, ka a Kɩrɩsɩto ɩ̃gãn na tʋ̃ɔ mɛ.
49004013	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ na vɛ̃ ka sɩ jaa na ɩ bʋ̃'yen a sɔɔfʋ pɔ, na sɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, na sɩ baa tɩ ta a lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na be.
49004014	Sɩ kʋ̃ lɛ pãa chɛnɛ ɩ nɩtãa bibiir vavire yʋɔrɔ kɔ̃sɛbɛ kaar ɛ. Na sɩ ma dãdaal chen a puor nɩ a niem wiilfʋ jaa bʋrɔ nɩbɛ na de a ba yɛ̃ na ba bɛlɛ nɩ ɛ.
49004015	Tɩchɛ sɩn 'yɛrɛ na yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ nʋ̃fʋ na sɩn nʋ̃ɔn a yele a jaa pɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ a ju na ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto.
49004016	A wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa choofʋ jiir choo taa, naa tʋ̃ɔ nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nʋ̃fʋ pɔ, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tʋ̃nɔ̃ a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃.
49004017	Lɛ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ naa de a sɩ Soro yuor kpãkpãana ɩka, yɩ ta lɛ chɛnɛ maala fɩka a bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na maala turo nɩ a ba tɩɛr bur bur ɛ.
49004018	A ba tɩɛr lĩi naa ka baa pʋɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nyɛvʋr pɔ ɛ, bojũu a ba ba bɔ̃ɔfʋ yin a ba nyãkpɩ̃ɛn ban tara.
49004019	Ba ɩ naa ba bãma dẽme, na ba de a ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ pepe yele, na ba pãa irɛ a ala a jaa na ba vɩɛl ɛ, tɩ chɛnɛ bʋɔrɔ yaa.
49004020	Yɩn 'lɔ, a ba ɩ a sɔr nyã lɛ yɩ de bɔ̃ɔn a Kɩrɩsɩto ɛ.
49004021	Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ ɩka yɩn wõ a wʋ 'yɛr, ba wiil yɩ naa a yelmɩ̃ɛ na be a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ.
49004022	Ba wiil yɩ naa a lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ maala ɩka, yɩ yaa a kõr maalfʋ 'lɔ bar na bɛl yɩ nɩ a wʋ vɔlaa,
49004023	tɩ na yɩ ɩ nɩpaalaa a yɩ befʋ nɩ a yɩ tɩɛr pɔ.
49004024	Yɩ de a be paalaa 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na maal a wʋ kaar na yɩ su, a ɩ naa yelmɩ̃ɛ torfʋ nɩ chɛchɛ.
49004025	A lɛ jũu, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ bar jir ŋmaafʋ tɩ 'yɛrɛ yelmɩ̃ɛ kʋrɔ a wʋ taaba, bojũu sɩ jaa ben a ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen pɔ,
49004026	"Fʋ̃ʋ wa nyɛ suur taa maal dɛɛr ɛ." Ta vɛ̃ ka a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ mʋr pɔɔ fʋ nɩ a suur ɛ.
49004027	Yɩ taa yuoro sɔr kʋrɔ a Satan a wʋ bɛl yɩ ɛ.
49004028	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ juro, wʋ ta ma lɛ juro ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ma tʋ̃nɔ̃ tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala na tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a wʋ nuur na wʋ nyɛ bʋ̃kɔ̃ɔ, na wʋ ir sʋ̃ʋn a nɔ̃n dẽme.
49004029	Yɩ taa vɛ̃ ka a 'yɛr sɔ̃ɔnsɩ yire a yɩ nɛɛr pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ 'yɛrsɩ ala na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yɩ taaba ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn ala ɩ yele kɔ̃ɔ fɛr ba naa, naa mɩ ɩ sʋ̃ʋfʋ kʋ a bala na chɛlɛ.
49004030	Na yɩ taa vɛ̃ ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, 'lɔ wʋn de 'yɔ̃ɔn yɩ a jɩ̃nɛ gun a faafʋ bɩbir.
49004031	Yɩ ir putuo, pʋɔm 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, nɩ suur, tãn taa, nɩ tʋfʋ, nɩ 'laarfʋ 'yɛrbie.
49004032	Yɩ maala vɩla na yɩ kaara taa nɩbaal, na yɩ vɛ̃nɛ kʋrɔ taa nɩtãa lɛ Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃ kʋ yɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto jũu.
49005001	Yɩ tɔɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn an ɩ yɩ ɩ naa a wʋ binʋ̃nsɩ,
49005002	na yɩ kpɩɛrɛ nɩ nʋ̃fʋ nɩtãa lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na nʋ̃ sɩ na wʋ de a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ maal a sɩ bɔɔrlo bon na nyuro vɩla lon a bɔɔr ka a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ pɛl.
49005003	Tɩchɛ a yɩ pɔ, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka ba wa pʋr sɛ̃sɛ̃yele, bɩɩ folaa ɩfʋ, bɩɩ bɔgarfʋ ɛ, bojũu a anyãna ba sɛɛn a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ chɛchɛsɩ ɛ.
49005004	Yɩ taa lɛ 'yɛrɛ vɩ̃ 'yɛrbie ɛ, bɩɩ jɔl 'yɛr, bɩɩ jɔl dɩ̃ɛn ɛ, ala po naa, tɩchɛ yɩ dãna Nãaŋmɩn.
49005005	Bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a anyãna sɩrɛ jaa ɩka nɩrɛ na sɛ̃nɛ, nɩfolaa, bɔgar sʋɔ, wʋ ɩ naa nɩrɛ na puoro tɩbɛ, na wʋ kʋ̃ nyɛ jie be a Kɩrɩsɩto nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ ɛ.
49005006	Yɩ taa vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa bɛl yɩ nɩ 'yɛr pɔrsɩ ɛ, bojũu anyãna lɛ so ka Nãaŋmɩn su tuo waara a bawõnsɩ jie.
49005007	A lɛ jũu yɩ taa mara ba ɛ.
49005008	Bojũu yɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ libe, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã yɩ ɩ naa chãa a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ. Yɩ kpɩɛrɛ nɩtãa a chãa bibiir.
49005009	A chãa wɔ̃mɔ̃ ɩ naa vɩla maalfʋ, yeltorsɩ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
49005010	Yɩ mɔ̃ na yɩ jãn a ala na pɛlɛ a sɩ Soro pʋɔ.
49005011	Na yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa pʋɔrɔ a libe tʋ̃mɔ̃ na ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ yin naa chãa pɔ.
49005012	Bojũu a gba ma ɩrɛ na vɩ̃ a ala a bawõnsɩ na ma maala a libe pɔ manfʋ.
49005013	Tɩchɛ bon jaa wa yi chãa pɔ, fʋ ma nyɛn wʋn chaar.
49005014	Bojũu chãa lɛ ma vɛ̃ ka fʋ nyɛ bon jaa chɛchɛ. Ala lɛ so a ba 'yɛr, "A fʋ̃ʋ gʋ̃ɔ sʋɔ, jɛɔ ir a kũu pɔ, ka a Kɩrɩsɩto chaar 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ."
49005015	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃ a lɛ yɩn kpɩɛrɛ, ka a ta ɩ jɔl kpɛfʋ tɩchɛ ka a ɩ yɛ̃ kpɛfʋ.
49005016	Na yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir yɩn wa nyɛ jie ka wʋ ta sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, bojũu a bɩbie anyãna ba vɩɛlɛ ɛ.
49005017	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta ɩ jɔlɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a ala a sɩ Soro na bʋɔrɔ.
49005018	Yɩ ta nyũ dãa buu ɛ, an sɔ̃ɔ yɩn ju, tɩ yɩ vɛ̃ ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛɛ yɩ.
49005019	Na yɩ yiele a Nãaŋmɩn yiel nɩ a ala na ɩ a Sɩɛ yiel kʋrɔ taa, na yɩ yiele dãnfʋ yiel nɩ a yɩ nyãa wʋ jaa kʋrɔ a sɩ Soro.
49005020	Yɩ ma dãna a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn yele a jaa pɔ, nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor.
49005021	Yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ taa a Kɩrɩsɩto yɩn 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ jũu.
49005022	Pɔbɔ, yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a yɩ sɩrbɛ, nɩtãa lɛ yɩn siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a sɩ Soro.
49005023	Bojũu an ɩ a sɩrɛ lɛ ɩ a pɔɔ ju, nɩtãa lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a pupuorbiir ju, na ɩ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn na wʋ ɩ a Fafaara.
49005024	A lɛ jũu, lɛ a pupuorbiir na siir a ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Kɩrɩsɩto, lɛ lɛ a pɔbɔ mɩ, yɩ siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a yɩ sɩrbɛ yele a jaa pɔ.
49005025	Sɩrbɛ, yɩ nʋ̃ a yɩ pɔbɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na nʋ̃ a pupuorbiir na wʋ de a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ ba,
49005026	wʋ maal ban a lɛ ka ban ɩ chɛchɛ, na wʋ de kʋ̃ɔ pɛɛn ba ka ba vɩɛlɛ nɩ a 'yɛr.
49005027	Wʋ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ de a pupuorbiir banyã na vɩɛlɛ kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, na waa tara jɩ̃nɛ ɛ, 'mabfʋ jie ɛ, bɩɩ dɛɛr jie jaa ɛ, tɩchɛ a ba ɩ chɛchɛ ba tara yele jaa ɛ.
49005028	A lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a yɩn sɩrbɛ, yɩ nʋ̃ a yɩ pɔbɔ, nɩtãa lɛ yɩn nʋ̃ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɩ̃gãma. A 'lɔ na nʋ̃ a wʋ pɔɔ nʋ̃n a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
49005029	Nɩrɛ jaa ba be na 'laar a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɩ̃gãn ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ma kʋrɔ wʋn bʋ̃diir na wʋ kaara wʋ, lɛ lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto kaara a pupuorbiir.
49005030	Bojũu sɩ ɩ naa a wʋ ɩ̃gãn jiir,
49005031	"A lɛ jũu, daba na bar a wʋ sãa nɩ a wʋ ma, tɩchɛ ka 'lɔ nɩ a wʋ pɔɔ ɩ bʋ̃'yen, ka ba jaa ayi ɩ ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃'yen."
49005032	A anyã ɩ naa a 'yɛr sɔɔlaa, tɩchɛ maa 'yɛrɛ naa a Kɩrɩsɩto nɩ a pupuorbiir 'yɛr.
49005033	A yɩn mɩ gba, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ ma nʋ̃ a wʋ pɔɔ nɩtãa lɛ wʋn nʋ̃ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, ka a pɔɔ mɩ ma 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wʋ sɩrɛ.
49006001	Bibiir, yɩn be a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ, yɩ wõnõ a yɩ dɔɔrbɔ toor, a lɛ lɛ tor.
49006002	A lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ kʋ a wʋ nɛɛ, a nɛɛ nyã lɛ ɩ a nɛdɔ̃ɔ wʋn tɩr, "'Yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ sãa nɩ a fʋ ma,
49006003	an ɩn vɩla kʋ fʋ, a fʋ wõ nʋ̃ɔ kor ka a wɛr pɔ."
49006004	Sãamɩne yɩ taa maala a yɩ bibiir ka ba nyɛrɛ suur ɛ, tɩ yɩ guolo ba, na yɩ jãna ba, wile nɩ ba a ala na yi a sɩ Soro sɛ̃.
49006005	Gbãgbaar yɩ wõnõ a yɩ sorbo toor na yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba tɩ joro ba nɩ a yɩ pʋpɛl nɩtãa lɛ yɩn wõnõ a Kɩrɩsɩto toor.
49006006	Yɩ wõnõ a ba toor ka a ta ɩ ban fur nɩbir 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ir nyãa 'yɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ yɩn ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto gbãgbaar na yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ.
49006007	Yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ pʋpɛl fɩka a sɩ Soro Yesu yɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ, a ta ɩ nɩsaal lɛ ɛ.
49006008	Bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a sɩ Soro na yab ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa lɛ wʋn tʋ̃ a vɩla jɩ̃, ka gbãgbaa lɛ wʋ ɩ bɩɩ waa ɩ gbãgbaa ɛ.
49006009	A yɩn sorbo, yɩ mɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ nɛ kʋrɔ a yɩ gbãgbaar. Yɩ ta pirpire ba ɛ, na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka a 'lɔ na ɩ a ba Soro mɩ lɛ ɩ a yɩ Soro na wʋ be a saaju, 'lɔ lɛ ba turo nʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ.
49006010	A baaraa lɛ ɩka yɩ kpɛ̃mɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩ a wʋ tʋ̃ɔfʋ kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ.
49006011	Yɩ de a Nãaŋmɩn tãjɛbonsɩ a jaa su na yɩ tʋ̃ɔ ara jɛb a tɩɩ nɛbɛr.
49006012	Bojũu a ba ɩ sɩn nɩ nɩsaal lɛ jɛɛrɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩ jɛɛrɛ nɩ naa a sɩɩr tʋ̃ɔfʋ dẽme, nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, nɩ a wɛr nyã libe kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ ala na be a saaju.
49006013	A lɛ jũu, yɩ de a Nãaŋmɩn tãjɛbonsɩ a jaa su, ka a bɩbir bier 'lɔ wa vɩɛ, ka yɩ ba gbɛr, na yɩ tʋ̃ɔ jɛb a jɛɛr baar tɩ na yɩ chɛnɛ ara.
49006014	Yɩ pãa ara kpɛ̃ɔ, na yɩ de a yelmɩ̃ɛ ka wʋ ɩ a sɩɛ gãn a yɩ sɛ, na yɩ de torfʋ ka wʋ ɩ a nyãa wɩɛ,
49006015	na yɩ 'mi'mine a nyã'maar 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ 'yɛrfʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a ɩ a yɩ gbɛɛ nafɔɔr.
49006016	A 'lɔ na pʋɔ a jaa pɔ nɩ nyã ɩka, yɩ de a yɩ bʋ̃piiraa na ɩ a yɩ sɔɔfʋ na yɩ tʋ̃ɔ de kpĩin a dɛɛr sʋɔ pĩme na 'lɩrɛ.
49006017	Yɩ de a kur jupil su, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a yɩ faafʋ, nɩ a sɔkpɛ̃ɛ na yi a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɛ̃, na wʋ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr.
49006018	Na yɩ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn lɛ a wʋ Sɩɛ na wiil yɩ sɔ̃ɔ jaa, nɩ sʋɔrfʋ jaa bʋrɔ. Yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir jʋrɔ na yɩ sʋɔrɔ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ a wʋ nɩbɛ ba jaa.
49006019	Yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ ma, ka maa wa haara a nɛɛ, ka Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ma a wʋ 'yɛrbie ka n taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩ na n 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã yelsɔɔlaa.
49006020	A Yesu 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã ɩn ara kʋ jũu lɛ so, ka ba 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ. Yɩ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ ma ka n taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩ 'yɛrɛ a lɛ na sɛɛ.
49006021	Tɩchɩkusɩ na ɩ a yɛbɛ nʋ̃ naa na wʋ tara yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a sɩ Soro tʋ̃mɔ̃. Wʋn man yele jaa kʋ yɩ, ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ ɩn be nɩ a lɛ ɩn ma maala.
49006022	A anyãna jũu lɛ n tʋ̃n wʋ a yɩ sɛ̃, ka yɩn bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ sɩn be tɩ na wʋ mɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
49006023	Nyã'maar wʋ be a yɩn na ɩ a yɛɛr sɛ̃, nɩ nʋ̃fʋ lɔ̃ɔn sɔɔfʋ na yi a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃.
49006024	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋ be a bala jaa na nʋ̃ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃ nɩ nʋ̃fʋ 'lɔ na ba baaraa ɛ.
50001001	Maa Pɔɔl nɩ Timoti na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ, lɛ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ be a Filipai, lɔ̃ɔn a pupuorbiir nɩdierbe nɩ a sʋ̃sʋ̃nbɔ.
50001002	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃, a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
50001003	N ma puor a n Nãaŋmɩn yãan, maa wa tɩɛr yɩ sɔ̃ɔ jaa.
50001004	N ma sʋɔrɔ na Nãaŋmɩn nɩ pʋpɛl kʋrɔ a yɩ jaa a n Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ pɔ,
50001005	bojũu yɩ mɩ pʋɔ man mʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbir tɔtaa a bɩbir dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, tɩ tãn a pʋ̃pãanyã.
50001006	A nɩtɔ̃ jũu, n tara na sɔɔfʋ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na piel a tʋ̃vɩla a yɩ pɔ, na kãan ka a tɩ baar a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto waa bɩbir.
50001007	A tara na sɔr ɩka n tɩɛr a nɩtɔ̃ a yɩ jaa jũu, ɩn tara a yɩ tɩɛr jũu, ka ba lũ man nɩ bɔ̃jɔrsɩ bɩɩ, baa lũ ma ɛ, n chɛnɛ na mana a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɩka a ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ, yɩ jaa lɔ̃ɔ põn ma a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ.
50001008	Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ɩ a n dãasɩɛ sʋɔ a lɛ ɩn tara a yɩ tɩɛr fɩka a lɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na tara a yɩ tɩɛr.
50001009	Maa Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ nɩ nyã ɩka, a yɩ nʋ̃ taa wʋ lɛ pʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ jaa, nɩ yɛ̃ nɩ par bɔ̃ɔfʋ.
50001010	Yɩn wa ɩrɛ a lɛ, an sʋ̃ʋ yɩ na ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ bon 'lɔ na ɩ bʋ̃sʋ̃, ka a Kɩrɩsɩto waa bɩbir, ka yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ tɩ na yɩ ta tara chɛfʋ jaa ɛ,
50001011	na yɩn sɛɛn yeltorsɩ wɔ̃mɔ̃ tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ, ka nɩbɛ pɛɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn yuor tɩɩr.
50001012	N yɛɛr, n bʋɔrɔ na ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a par ɩka a lɛ na ɩ a n sɛ̃, sʋ̃ʋ ma naa ka n mʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbir.
50001013	A lɛ na ɩ jũu, a chaar kʋ a bala na guro a nãa yir nɩ nɩrɛ jaa ɩka, ba 'yɔ̃ɔ ma naa a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto jũu.
50001014	A maa ban 'yɔ̃ɔ a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ jũu, a yɛɛr yɔɔ jie na tara sɔɔfʋ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ chɛnɛ na tara ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ mʋɔlɔ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nɩ nyãa ba joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
50001015	A ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka, nɩbɛ bamɩne mʋɔlɔ na a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yele ban tara nɩ ma nyuur nɩ nɛchɩrɛ jũu, tɩchɛ bamɩne 'lɔ, mʋɔlɔ na a Kɩrɩsɩto yele na sʋ̃ʋn ma.
50001016	Banyãna lɛ mʋɔlɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto yele yin nʋ̃fʋ pɔ, na ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɩka ba pɔɔ ma naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbir mʋɔlfʋ jũu.
50001017	A bala ɩn de nie 'yɛr a ba 'yɛr na mʋɔl a 'yɛr nɩ nyuur, maal a lɛ ɩka a n dɔɔyɛ wʋ lɛ pʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ.
50001018	Tɩchɛ bo lɛ an ɩ? A lɛ na ɩ nɩbijɩɛ lɛ ɩka ba mʋɔl a Yesu yele sɔr jaa pɔ, ka ba sɔɔn ɩka yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ bɩɩ, jire lɛ bɩɩ, a nɩtɔ̃ vɛ̃ naa ka n pʋɔ pɛl. Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa ɩn chɛnɛ na tara pʋpɛl.
50001019	Bojũu n bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka tu a yɩ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ nɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto Sɩɛ sʋ̃ʋfʋ jũu, a lɛ na ɩ a n sɛ̃ ɩn nyɛn faafʋ.
50001020	Bon 'lɔ na ɩ ma nɩbijɩɛ nɩ a n tɩɛrtɔ jie lɛ ɩka, vɩ̃ wʋ ta kpɛ ma sɔr jaa pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka n tara ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ ka a Kɩrɩsɩto na nyɛ tɩɩr a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a n nyɛvʋr pɔ lɛ, bɩɩ a n kũu pɔ lɛ.
50001021	Bojũu maa 'lɔ, maa chɛnɛ nyɛvʋr pɔ, n ben be kʋ a Kɩrɩsɩto, ka maa mɩ kpi, ka a ɩ tɔ̃nɔ̃.
50001022	Ala ɩ n chɛnɛ na nyɛvʋr pɔ, ɩn tʋ̃n tʋ̃vɩɛl yɔɔ, tɩchɛ n kaa ir buor? N ba bɔ̃ɔ a 'lɔ ɩn na kaa ir ɛ.
50001023	A yelsɩ ayi anyã lũ ma naa, maa bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka n yi a ka tɩ be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃. A lɛ lɛ vɩla,
50001024	tɩchɛ a chɛnɛ na fɛr kʋ yɩ, ala ɩ ɩn chɛnɛ na a nyɛvʋr pɔ.
50001025	Ɩn be na bɔ̃ɔn a nɩtɔ̃, n bɔ̃ɔn na yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa ɩka ɩn chɛnɛ na be a yɩ jaa sɛ̃ naa sʋ̃nɔ̃ yɩ ka yɩ sɔɔ Nãaŋmɩn, na yɩ tara pʋpɛl a yɩn sɔɔ wʋ jũu.
50001026	A lɛ ɩn lɛ lɛ be a yɩ sɛ̃ go, ka a yɩ pʋpɛl yɩn tara a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ pʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ jũu.
50001027	Yele jaa wa ɩ, yɩ nyɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ vɩla a lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ na wile. Ka n wan wa nyɛ yɩ bɩɩ, maa ba wa be a yɩ sɛ̃ tɩ wõ a yɩ yele, ɩn bɔ̃ɔn ɩka yɩ ara na kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen, na yɩ tara tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen a sɔɔfʋ nɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ pɔ,
50001028	na yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bala na 'yɛr ɩka a ba ɩ lɛ lɛ ɛ. A nyã ɩn jɩ̃nɛ kʋ ba ɩka ban din dɔɔyɛ, tɩchɛ ka Nãaŋmɩn faa yɩ.
50001029	'Lɔ lɛ kʋ yɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu, a ba ɩ a Yesu yɩn sɔɔ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩn lɔ̃ɔn wʋ dire a dɔɔyɛ jũu.
50001030	Ka a dɔɔyɛ nyã yɩn be na dire ɩn a dɔɔyɛ 'lɔ yɩn nyɛ ɩn di, nɩ a dɔɔyɛ yɩn be na chɛnɛ wõnõ ɩn dire.
50002001	Ala ɩ yɩ tara na ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ, bojũu yɩ ɩn bʋ̃'yen nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto, na yɩ tara ɩ̃gãn 'maar a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ pɔ, na yɩ tara nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na yɩ nyɛ vɩla nɩ nɩbaal,
50002002	yɩ pãa vɛ̃n ka a n pʋpɛl sɛɛ, yɩn tara tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen, na yɩ tara nʋ̃fʋ bʋ̃'yen, na yɩ tara Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ bʋ̃'yen nɩ tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen.
50002003	Yɩ ta maal yele 'lɔ na ɩ nyuur yele bɩɩ na yɩ wile yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩbɛ gar a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ.
50002004	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ ta bʋɔrɔ a wʋ pʋpɛl bonsɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ ala nɩ na pɛlɛ a yɩ taaba pʋʋr.
50002005	Yɩ tara a tɩɛr nyã nɩ wʋ ju a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na dɔ̃ɔ tara.
50002006	Wʋn sɔɔ jɩ̃taa nɩ Nãaŋmɩn ka ba ɩ bʋ̃'yen, tɩchɛ waa de a jɩ̃taa nyã mana nɩ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, wʋ den bar,
50002007	tɩchɛ na wʋ siir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, na wʋ maal wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃, ka ba dɔɔ wʋ ka wʋ tara nɩsaal ɩ̃gãn, na wʋ ɩ nɩsaal.
50002008	Wʋ siir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩsaal kaar tu a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ kpin a daa ju.
50002009	A lɛ jũu, Nãaŋmɩn 'mɔɔ wʋn ka wʋ do gar bon jaa, na wʋ kʋ wʋ yuor na gar a yoe a jaa.
50002010	Nãaŋmɩn maal a nɩtɔ̃ ka a Yesu yuor jũu, gbɛdumo jaa na gbur naa a saaju nɩ a wɛr pɔ, nɩ a tẽe par,
50002011	ka a jãlbie a jaa 'yɛr ɩka, Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ ɩ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn yuor tɩɩr.
50002012	A lɛ jũu, n yɛɛr, nɩtãa a lɛ jaa yɩn ma sɔɔ ma, a ba ɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn maa wa be a yɩ jie tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ sɔɔ ma gar a lɛ ɩn sɔɔ ba be a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ. Yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir tʋ̃nɔ̃ a yɩ faafʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ dãbɩ̃ɛ nɩ mɩrfʋ.
50002013	Bojũu yɩn tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ a lɛ an ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ sʋ̃nɔ̃ yɩ ka yɩ tara ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ na yɩn tʋ̃ a lɛ wʋ̃n bʋɔrɔ.
50002014	Yɩ ma maal bon jaa tɩ na yɩ ta ma ɩrɛ gbʋrɔ̃ gbʋrɔ̃ bɩɩ chɩrɛ taa ɛ.
50002015	Ka yɩ kʋ̃ tara chɛfʋ nɩ yele jaa ɛ, na yɩ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bibiir banyã na ba tara chɛfʋ jaa ɛ, na yɩ kpɩɛrɛ wɛr nyã pɔ tʋ̃dɛbɛ nɩ yelbe-ɩrbɛ na be na yɩ chaar ŋmɛrbie kaar a wɛr pɔ.
50002016	A lɛ yɩn sɔɔ a nyɛvʋr 'yɛr lɛ na sʋ̃ʋ ma ka a Yesu waa bɩbir ka n na tʋ̃ɔ wiil a n mɩ̃ɛ ɩka n ba jo pɔrɔ ɛ, bɩɩ a n tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba ɩ pɔrɔ ɛ.
50002017	Ala sɔɔ ɩ ɩn din dɔɔyɛ naa pʋɔ a yɩ dɔɔyɛ pɔ yɩn dire yɩn sɔɔ Nãaŋmɩn jũu, n pʋɔ pɛl naa nɩ yɩ jaa.
50002018	A lɛ jũu, yɩ mɩ pʋɔ ma ka sɩ chɩlɛ.
50002019	Ala ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu wa sɔɔ naa, ɩn tʋ̃n Timoti ka wʋ wa a yɩ sɛ̃ sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ ka n wõ a yɩ yele ka a ɩ̃gãn 'maa ma.
50002020	N ba tara nɩrɛ jaa na kaara a wʋ kaar ɛ, ka wʋ na tara a yɩ bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ jaa ɛ.
50002021	Ba jaa bʋɔrɔ naa a ba pʋpɛl bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ, na baa bʋɔrɔ ala na pɛlɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pʋɔ ɛ.
50002022	Tɩchɛ Timoti tɩɛr 'lɔ yɩn bɔ̃ɔn fɩka sãa nɩ wʋ bie, wʋ pʋɔ ma naa ka sɩ mʋɔl a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ.
50002023	A lɛ jũu, n bʋɔrɔ na ɩka n tʋ̃ wʋ a yɩ sɛ̃, maa wa nyɛ lɛ yelsɩ na ɩrɛ kʋrɔ ma.
50002024	N sɔɔ naa ɩka a sɩ Soro na yuon sɔr kʋ ma ka maa mɩ̃ɛ wa nyɛ yɩ fɔɔ jaa.
50002025	Bojũu n nyɛn ka a ɩ fɛrfʋ kʋ ma ɩka n tʋ̃ Epafaroditusɩ na ɩ a n yɛbɛ nɩ a n tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ sʋɔ, na wʋ mɩ dire a n dɔɔyɛ tɔ sʋɔ. Wʋ mɩ ɩn a yɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ yɩn tʋ̃ ka wʋ wa maal a n bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ kʋ ma.
50002026	Bojũu wʋ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka wʋ nyɛ yɩ jaa tɩchɛ ka a wʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ jaa, bojũu yɩ wõn an ɔɔrɔ wʋ.
50002027	Yelmɩ̃ɛ, a ɔɔrɔ wʋn nɩbijɩɛ ka wʋ chɛ bɩ̃lãa naa kpi. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn wa kãan a wʋ nɩbaal, a ba ɩ 'lɔ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ mɩ kãan a n nɩbaal, ka n ta tara pʋsɔ̃ɔ yɔɔ ɛ.
50002028	Bojũu maa lɛ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir ɩka n tʋ̃ wʋ a yɩ sɛ̃, ka a yɩ pʋɔ na pɛl ala ɩ yɩ lɛ nyɛ wʋn go, ka a n ɩ̃gãn na 'maa.
50002029	Yɩ sɔɔ de wʋ nɩ pʋpɛl a sɩ Soro jũu, na yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nɩbɛ banyã taaba,
50002030	bojũu wʋ din dɔɔyɛ a wʋ nyɛvʋr pɔ, na wʋ ta ɩrɛ na kpi a Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃mɔ̃ jũu ɩka wʋ tʋ̃ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala yɩn ba tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃ kʋ ma ɛ.
50003001	N yɛɛr, a baaraa nɩ nyã ɩka yɩ tara pʋpɛl a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ. A ba ɩ tuo kʋ ma ɩn lɛ sɛɛrɛ a yelsɩ ala nɩ a ju kʋrɔ yɩ go ɛ, an ɩn sʋ̃ʋfʋ kʋ yɩ.
50003002	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃ nɩ a baar banyãna, ba ɩn yelbe-ɩrbɛ na ba ma ŋmara nɩbɛ yɔɩ pɔrɔ.
50003003	Bojũu sɩn lɛ ɩ a yɔŋmarba sɩrɛ jaa, na sɩ puoro a Nãaŋmɩn a Sɩɛ pɔ, na sɩ tara tɩɩr a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, na saa kaara a ɩ̃gãn ɛ.
50003004	Maa gba tara na mana na tʋ̃ɔ man tu a ɩ̃gãn pɔ. Ala ɩ nɩrɛ mɩ tara na yelsɩ amɩne na man, ka a lɛ na vɛ̃ ka wʋ tara sɔɔfʋ a ɩ̃gãn pɔ, maa tara na gar wʋ.
50003005	Ba ŋmaan a n yʋɔr a ber aniin daar, ka n ɩ a Isɩral nɩrɛ naa ɩ a Benjamin bal nɩrɛ, naa ɩ Heburu, ka ba dɔɔ ma ka ɩ Heburu nɩrɛ. A nɛɛ tufʋ jũu, ka ɩ Farasee.
50003006	N dɔ̃ɔn mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir naa gere a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ, a nɛbinãa yeltorsɩ jũu, n ba tara chɛfʋ jaa ɛ.
50003007	Tɩchɛ a ala a jaa ɩn dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ tɩɛr ɩka a tara na tɔ̃nɔ̃, n wa nyɛn ka a ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ jaa kʋ ma ɛ, a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jũu.
50003008	Bo lɛ gar a nɩtɔ̃, n nyɛn ka bon jaa ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, maa de man ala na tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ala ɩ n bɔ̃ɔ naa a n Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a tɩɩr sʋɔ. A wʋ jũu lɛ n bar bonsɩ a jaa. A ɩn sɔ̃sɔɔr kʋ ma, ɩn bʋɔrɔ ɩka n bɔ̃ɔ Kɩrɩsɩto,
50003009	tɩ naa bʋɔrɔ ɩka n be a wʋ pɔ, naa ta bʋɔrɔ a maa mɩ̃ɛ yeltorsɩ ala na yi a nɛbinãa pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yeltorsɩ ala na yi a Kɩrɩsɩto sɔɔfʋ pɔ. A yeltorsɩ anyã lɛ yi Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ naa ɩ sɔɔfʋ.
50003010	N bʋɔrɔ na ɩka n bɔ̃ɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto nɩ a wʋ kũu pɔ lɩɛb irfʋ kpɛ̃ɔ, naa lɔ̃ɔn wʋ di a dɔɔyɛ wa kaara a wʋ kaar a wʋ kũu pɔ,
50003011	ka n mɩ wa pʋɔ a bala mɩ na wa lɩɛb ir a kũu pɔ.
50003012	A ba ɩ n tara na a anyãna a jaa ɛ, bɩɩ n ɩn chɛchɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ n mʋ̃ɔn nɩbir ɩka n nyɔɔ kpɛ̃ɔ, ka Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ nyɔɔ ma kpɛ̃ɔ.
50003013	N yɛɛr, n ba 'yɛr ɩka n nyɔɔn yele jaa baar ɛ. Tɩchɛ yele bʋ̃'yen ɩn ɩ lɛ ɩka, n ĩin a ala na be a puor bar, tɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir tɩɛrɛ a ala na be a niem.
50003014	N mʋ̃ɔn nɩbir ɩka n tɩ de a saaju kʋfʋ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl ma tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
50003015	A sɩn bala na baa a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pɔ, sɩ mɩ ma tara a bonsɩ a nyãna tɩɛr. Tɩ yɩn wa tɩɛr yelyuo yele jaa pɔ, Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃n ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a yelnyɩnɛ.
50003016	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka sɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a bonsɩ anyãna sɩn ben tara.
50003017	N yɛɛr, yɩ pʋɔ a yɩ taaba na yɩ turo a lɛ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ maal wiil yɩ, na yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a bala na kpɩɛrɛ a lɛ sɩn wiil yɩ.
50003018	Bojũu n dɔ̃ɔ de nie 'yɛr kʋ yɩ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã nɩbikʋ̃ɔ pɔ lɛ n 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, bamɩne kpɩɛrɛ na fɩka a Kɩrɩsɩto daa ɩn 'laarfʋ kʋ ba.
50003019	A ba baaraa ɩn sɔ̃ɔfʋ, a ba ŋmɩn lɛ ɩ a ba ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ. Ba wile na ba mɩ̃ɛ nɩ yelsɩ ala na ɩ vɩ̃ nɩ ɩfʋ, a ba tɩɛrsɩ ɩn a wɛr nyã ju bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ tɛɛ tɩɛr.
50003020	Tɩchɛ sɩn 'lɔ ɩn saaju Nãaŋmɩn bibiir, be lɛ sɩ chɛlɛ a Fafaara na ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ka wʋ na yi wa.
50003021	A 'lɔ na tara kpɛ̃ɔ tʋ̃ɔ bon jaa na wʋ pire, wʋn den a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ lɩɛb a sɩ ɩ̃gãma ka a kaara a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩɩr ɩ̃gãn kaar.
50004001	A lɛ jũu, n yɛɛr yɩn ɩn nʋ̃, naa pãa bʋɔrɔ ɩka n nyɛ yɩ, yɩn lɛ ɩ a n pʋpɛl nɩ a nãa jupil, yɩ ara kpɛ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro pɔ n barmɩne.
50004002	N 'maal a Yuodiya nɩ Sɩntachi ɩka ba tara a tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen nyãna a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ.
50004003	Ɔ̃ɔ, n mɩ lɛ sʋɔrɔ fʋ naa, n baraa ɩka fʋ sʋ̃ʋ a pɔbɔ banyãna, ba lɔ̃ɔn man di dɔɔyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ mʋɔlfʋ pɔ 'matãan Kɩlɛmɛntɩ, na ɩ a n tʋ̃tʋ̃taaba, a bala yoe na be a nyɛvʋr gãn pɔ.
50004004	Yɩ tara pʋpɛl a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ sɔ̃ɔ jaa. N lɛ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ, yɩ tara pʋpɛl.
50004005	Vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa nyɛ lɛ yɩn siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ jɩ̃. A sɩ Soro waa ta naa.
50004006	Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka yele jaa wõnõ yɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yɩ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ pɔ, yɩ ma puor wʋ yãan, na yɩ vɛ̃ ka Nãaŋmɩn bɔ̃ɔ a bon 'lɔ yɩn bʋɔrɔ.
50004007	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã'maar na gar a nɩsaal bɔ̃ɔfʋ, na gun a yɩ nyãn, nɩ a yɩ tɩɛrsɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
50004008	N yɛɛr, a baaraa nɩ nyã ɩka bon 'lɔ jaa na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, nɩ bon 'lɔ jaa na ɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, nɩ bon 'lɔ jaa na tor, nɩ bon 'lɔ jaa na ɩ chɛchɛ, bon 'lɔ jaa na ɩ nʋ̃fʋ, nɩ bon 'lɔ jaa na ɩ pʋpɛl, ala ɩ bon 'lɔ jaa na ɩ vɩla, nɩ bon 'lɔ jaa na sɛɛn pɛɛfʋ, yɩ tɩɛrɛ a bonsɩ anyãna.
50004009	Bon jaa yɩn jãn tɩ na yɩ nyɛ, tɩ na yɩ wõ yi a n sɛ̃, yɩ maala yaa, ka a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ nyã'maar sʋɔ, na ben a yɩ sɛ̃.
50004010	N tara na pʋpɛl a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩ yɩn wiil ɩka yɩ chɛnɛ na tara a n tɩɛr. Yelmɩ̃ɛ yɩ dɔ̃ɔ tara a n tɩɛr tɩ na yaa tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ sɔr wiil ɛ.
50004011	N ba 'yɛrɛ wile ɩka n bʋɔrɔ na bon jaa ɛ, bojũu n dɔ̃ɔ jãn lɛ ɩn na tara bon ka wʋ sɛɛn ma.
50004012	N bɔ̃ɔn lɛ an sɛɛ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ tara jaa pʋʋrbile, naa lɛ bɔ̃ɔ lɛ an sɛɛ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ tara yɔɔ. A yelsɔɔlaa nyãna lɛ n jãn naa guolo nɩ a n mɩ̃ɛ, ka kɔ̃ kpɛ man bɩɩ, ka n tara na na di bɩɩ, ka bɩ̃lãa gba lɛ n tara na di, ka n tara na yɔɔ bɩɩ, n ba tara bon jaa ɛ.
50004013	Ɩn tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a anyãna a jaa tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na kʋ ma a kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ.
50004014	Tɩchɛ yɩ maal vɩla, yɩn sʋ̃ʋ ma a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn dire a dɔɔyɛ.
50004015	Yɩn Filipai nɩbɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ jaa yɩn sɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa ɩn yi a Masedonɩya, pupuorbiir gbulsɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba kʋ ma bon ɛ, ka yɩn tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
50004016	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ gba ɩn be a Tɛsalonika, yɩ sʋ̃ʋ man nɩ a n bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ gar gbɛbʋ̃'yen.
50004017	A ba ɩ tɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ n bʋɔrɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ n bʋɔrɔ na ɩka yɩ nyɛ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn wʋ yab yɩ na wʋ sʋ̃ʋ yɩ.
50004018	N nyɛn a n sãyar yɔɔ, naa gba nyɛ tɩ põn bar ka a sɛɛn ma, pʋ̃pãanyã n nũu kpɛ naa a kʋfʋ ala yɩn tʋ̃n a Epafaroditusɩ ka wʋ wa kʋ ma, ka a yɩ kʋfʋ anyãna kaar fɩka a bɔɔrlo bomo ala na nyuro nʋ̃ɔ naa pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ.
50004019	A n Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ yɩn a yɩ bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ a jaa tu a wʋ tɩɩr nãbonsɩ ala na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
50004020	A sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn wʋ nyɛrɛ tɩɩr bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
50004021	Yɩ puor a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ba jaa na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ. A n yɛɛr na be a ka mɩ puoro yɩ naa.
50004022	A Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ mɩ ba jaa puoro yɩ naa, ka a bala mɩ na be a nãkpɛ̃ɛ Siisa yir mɩ puoro yɩ.
50004023	A sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ a be a yɩ sɩɩr pɔ. A ɩ a lɛ.
51001001	Maa Pɔɔl na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nãa an ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ pɔ nɩ Timoti na ɩ a sɩ yɛbɛ,
51001002	sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ nɩ a yɛɛr na tara a sɔɔfʋ a Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ na be a Kolose. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
51001003	Sɩ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan na ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto Sãa, sɩn wa sʋɔrɔ kʋrɔ yɩ,
51001004	bojũu sɩ wõn a yɩ sɔɔfʋ yɩn tara a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩ a nʋ̃fʋ 'lɔ yɩn tara kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ba jaa.
51001005	A yɩ sɔɔfʋ nɩ a nʋ̃fʋ na yi a tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie na gã gu yɩ be a saaju a 'lɔ yɩn de nie wõ, a yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr na ɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ
51001006	'lɔ na wa a yɩ sɛ̃. A wɛr wʋ jaa, a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã wɔ̃nɔ̃ na wɔ̃mɔ̃ na a nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩtãa lɛ an ben ɩrɛ a yɩ pɔ, an yi a bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ daar jaa yɩn wõ naa na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ par a yelmɩ̃ɛ pɔ.
51001007	Yɩ jãn a nyã yin Epafaras sɛ̃ na ɩ a sɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ. Wʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ na de a sɩ jie mʋɔlɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr.
51001008	'Lɔ lɛ wa man kʋ sɩ a nʋ̃fʋ 'lɔ yɩn tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ pɔ.
51001009	A lɛ jũu, an yi a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ jaa sɩn wõ naa, saa dɔ̃ɔ gal ɩka sɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ yɩ ɛ, na sɩ sʋɔrɔ ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn wʋ pʋɔ yɩ a wʋ bɔfʋ yɛ̃, a sɩɛ pɔ yɛ̃, a jaa nɩ par bɔ̃ɔfʋ.
51001010	A sɩ sʋɔrfʋ lɛ ɩka, a yɩ befʋ a vɩɛlɛ kʋ a sɩ Soro, ka a pɛlɛ a wʋ pʋɔ, na yɩ wɔ̃nɔ̃ bisʋ̃n tʋ̃vɩla jaa pɔ, na yɩ baa a Nãaŋmɩn yɛ̃ pɔ.
51001011	Sɩ mɩ ma sʋɔrɔ na ɩka Nãaŋmɩn wʋ maal yɩ ka yɩ kpɛ̃mɛ nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn ala a jaa na yi a wʋ tɩɩr kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ, na yɩ nyɔɔrɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ tara kãnyir yele jaa pɔ, nɩ pʋpɛl.
51001012	Na yɩ ma dãna a Sãa, 'lɔ lɛ kaa a yɩ sɛɛ, ka yɩ na põ a Nãaŋmɩn nãbonsɩ nɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ a chãa pɔ.
51001013	Bojũu 'lɔ lɛ faa sɩ yin a libe kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ, na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ a wʋ Binʋ̃nãa nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
51001014	A wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ sɩ nyɛ faafʋ, na sɩ nyɛ yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ.
51001015	A Yesu na wa tɩ wa a wɛr ju, 'lɔ lɛ wiil sɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã sɩn ba nyɛrɛ nɩ a nɩbir ɛ, a lɛ wʋn be. 'Lɔ lɛ tara kpɛ̃ɔ a bonsɩ a jaa pɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na maal.
51001016	Bojũu a wʋ pɔ lɛ a bonsɩ a jaa na be a saaju, nɩ a ala na be ka a wɛr pɔ maal, ala sɩn nyɛrɛ, nɩ a ala sɩn ba nyɛrɛ ɛ, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na tara kpɛ̃ɔ ɩ a tʋ̃ɔfʋ sʋɔ, nɩ a malakasɩ ala gba na tara kpɛ̃ɔ, nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn bonsɩ, a jaa maal tu a wʋ pɔ, ka a ɩ a wʋ sofʋ.
51001017	A 'lɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ a bonsɩ a jaa be be, a wʋ pɔ lɛ a bonsɩ a jaa 'mataa.
51001018	'Lɔ mɩ lɛ ɩ a ɩ̃gãn ju sʋɔ, a pupuorbiir. 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ a pielfʋ, nɩ a bidɔ̃ɔ na wʋ de nie ir a kũu pɔ, na waa lɛ kpi go ɛ, ka yele jaa pɔ, ka wʋ ɩ a ju sʋɔ.
51001019	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ pɛl wʋ naa ka wʋ befʋ wʋ jaa be a wʋ pɔ.
51001020	A tun a wʋ pɔ, ka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ 'maal a bonsɩ a jaa kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, ka a ala na be a saaju bɩɩ a ala na be ka a wɛr pɔ. Wʋ maal ka nyã'maar be be, nɩ a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ a daa ju wʋn kpi.
51001021	Yɩ dɔ̃ɔ jãan a Nãaŋmɩn na yɩ ɩ a wʋ dɔ̃dẽme, a yɩ yeldɛbɛ ɩfʋ jũu.
51001022	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, wʋ 'maal yɩn tun a Kɩrɩsɩto na wa ɩ nɩsaal na wʋ kpi. Nãaŋmɩn maal a nɩtɔ̃ ka yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ a wʋ sɛ̃, na yɩ kʋ tara chɛfʋ jaa ɛ, bɩɩ tara 'yɛr dɔɔl ɛ,
51001023	ala ɩ yɩ chɛnɛ na ba gbɛr a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ, na yɩ taa tɔɔ yi a tɩɛrtɔ 'lɔ na ɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã yɩn wõ ɛ. A 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã lɛ yɩ wõ ban mʋɔl kʋ nɩrɛ jaa ka a wɛr ju. Ala lɛ a maa Pɔɔl ɩ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃.
51001024	Pʋ̃pãanyã, n pãa chɩlɛ naa a n dɔɔyɛ ɩn di a yɩ jũu, naa na di a dɔɔyɛ ala a jaa a Kɩrɩsɩto na bʋɔrɔ ɩka n di kʋ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn na ɩ a pupuorbiir jũu.
51001025	Nãaŋmɩn maal man ka n ɩ a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋ a pupuorbiir naa na man a wʋ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ jaa nɛ nɛ nɛ kʋ yɩ.
51001026	A yele nyãna lɛ sɔɔl a kõro jaa a sãakpãmɩne sɔ̃ɔ, tɩchɛ ka a pãa yi chãa pɔ a wʋ nɩbɛ sɛ̃.
51001027	Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kaa ir ɩka wʋ vɛ̃ ka a wʋ nɩbɛ bɔ̃ɔn sɩrɛ jaa a lɛ wʋ tara a tɩɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ ba jaa, ɩka a Kɩrɩsɩto ben a yɩ pɔ, na ɩ a tɩɩr tɩɛrtɔ jie.
51001028	A Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ sɩ mʋɔlɔ, na sɩ kpãana nɩrɛ jaa wile nɩ nɩrɛ jaa nɩ yɛ̃ jaa bʋrɔ, ka sɩ na de nɩrɛ jaa kʋ wʋ ka wʋ ɩ chɛchɛ.
51001029	A nyã jũu lɛ n tʋ̃nɔ̃ hãna dire dɔɔyɛ nɩ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ wʋ jaa wʋn tʋ̃nɔ̃ tun a n 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51002001	N bʋɔrɔ na ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ ɩn mʋɔrɔ a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩ a bala na be a Laodisea, nɩ a bala jaa na ba nyɛ a maa mɩ̃ɛ nɩ nɩbir ɛ.
51002002	Maa bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka yɩ tara ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn a yɩ nyãn pɔ, na yɩ ɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen nʋ̃ taa, ka a lɛ na vɛ̃ ka yɩ tara par bɔ̃ɔfʋ yɔɔ jaa a nãbonsɩ a jaa pɔ, na yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn yelsɔɔlsɩ, na ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto.
51002003	A wʋ pɔ lɛ a nãbonsɩ, nɩ a yɛ̃, nɩ a bɔ̃ɔfʋ a jaa sɔɔl.
51002004	N 'yɛrɛ na a nɩtɔ̃ kʋrɔ yɩ ka nɩrɛ jaa taa wa bɛl yɩ nɩ nɛchɩrɛ 'yɛr na nyɛtãan yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
51002005	An sɔɔ ɩ a maa mɩ̃ɛ na ba be a yɩ sɛ̃ gba ɛ, tɩchɛ n tara na a yɩ tɩɛr. N chɩlɛ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka n nyɛ a lɛ yɩn tara nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩ a lɛ a yɩ sɔɔfʋ na kpɛ̃mɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51002006	A lɛ jũu, yɩn de a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ka wʋ ɩ a Soro, yɩ chɛnɛ be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51002007	Yɩ ba nyɩbɛ na yɩ baa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, na yɩ nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ̃mɛ a sɔɔfʋ pɔ, fɩka a lɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ wiil yɩ, na yɩ ma puor wʋ yãan sɔ̃ɔ jaa.
51002008	Yɩ kaara sʋ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa ta wa de yɩ ka yɩ ɩ gbãgbaar tu a bɛlfʋ ala na ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ ɛ, nɩ nɩsaal yɛ̃ ɛ, na ɩ a ala na kaara a wɛr nyã ju ban taa kaara a Kɩrɩsɩto wiilfʋ.
51002009	A Nãaŋmɩn befʋ wʋ jaa ben a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51002010	Yɩ sɛɛ naa bojũu yɩ sɔɔn a Kɩrɩsɩto, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ tʋ̃ɔfʋ dẽme nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme ba jaa ju sʋɔ.
51002011	A wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ba mɩ ŋma yɩn a yɔɩ ka a yelbier 'lɔ na yi a yɩ pɔ, a ba ɩ yuor ŋmaafʋ 'lɔ nɩsaal na de wʋ nũu ŋmaan ɛ, tɩchɛ yʋɔr ŋmaafʋ 'lɔ Kɩrɩsɩto na ŋmaa.
51002012	Ban dɔ̃ɔ so yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ, ba ũu yɩn a Kɩrɩsɩto kaar, ka yɩ ir a kũu pɔ fɩka a Kɩrɩsɩto, bojũu yɩ sɔɔn de a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na sɩ̃ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto a kũu pɔ, na tara kpɛ̃ɔ.
51002013	Tɩchɛ a yɩn bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, sɛrɛ tɩ yɩ wa sɔɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto, yɩ dɔ̃ɔ kpi a yɩ sɩɩr pɔ, bojũu yɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ yelbe-ɩrbɛ, na yɩ jãan Nãaŋmɩn, bojũu yɩ sɔ̃ɔn a Nãaŋmɩn nɛbinsɩ. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ yɩn a nyɛvʋr paalaa a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, na wʋ vɛ̃ kʋ yɩ.
51002014	Nãaŋmɩn fɔfɔn a sɩ yelbebe ala na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb bin bar. Ala lɛ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr 'yɛr dɔɔl sɩ. Ala lɛ dɔ̃ɔ fɩrɛ sɩ na a ŋmaa sɩ yin, wʋ den bar na wʋ kpa yaa a daa ju.
51002015	Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃ɔn a sɩdɛbɛ nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, na wʋ maal ba ka a ɩ dãasɩɛ nɩyɔɔ jaa niem. Wʋ tʋ̃ɔ ba naa nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto daa ju kũu.
51002016	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa tɔɔr a yɩ 'yɛr nɩ bon 'lɔ yɩn dire bɩɩ nyuro ɛ, bɩɩ tun a Juu nɩbɛ lɔ̃ɔ difʋ pɔ ɛ, bɩɩ Chuu Paalaa Dɩ̃ɛn pɔ ɛ, bɩɩ a Pɛ̃nfʋ Bɩbir Daar ɛ.
51002017	A anyã ɩ naa a yelsɩ ala nɩ taa dɔ̃ɔ wa gãagiel, tɩchɛ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ben a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51002018	Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa kpãkpãan yɩ nɩ jir 'yɛr ɩka, yɩ siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ na yɩ puoro a malakasɩ ɛ, a lɛ na vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ kʋ̃ nyɛ a sãyar ɛ. A nɩrɛ nyã tɔ sʋɔ ma vɩɛr kpɛ a yele pɔ tɩɛr ɩka wʋ tara na kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ a ala wʋn nyɛ. A wʋ yelbier tɩɛr ma vɛ̃n ka wʋ wile wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
51002019	A nɩrɛ nyã ba nyɔɔ a 'lɔ na ɩ a ju ɛ. Nɩtãa a lɛ a ju na ma wile a ɩ̃gãn, ka a jile nʋ̃ɔ nyɔɔ a ɩ̃gãn 'mataa a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ.
51002020	An ɩ yɩn nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ 'mataa kpi, a wɛr nyã ju kpɩ̃ɛn bonsɩ, ba lɛ tara kpɛ̃ɔ a yɩ ju ɛ. Ŋmɩnɛ ka a yɩ kpɛfʋ chɛnɛ kaara fɩka yɩ chɛnɛ na ɩ a wɛr sofʋ?
51002021	Ta nyɔɔ bon nyã ɛ! Ta lɛm bon nyã kaa ɛ! Ta sɩɩr bon nyã kaa ɛ!
51002022	A nɛɛr anyãna a jaa tufʋ ɩn yelsɩ na ba lɛ tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ jaa ɛ, bojũu a ɩn nɩsaal nɛbinsɩ nɩ nɩsaal wiilfʋsɩ lɛ.
51002023	A nɛbinsɩ anyãna nyɛntãan fɩka yɛ̃ yele na ɩ a ba mɩ̃ɛ puorfʋ yele nɩ mɩ̃ɛ siirfʋ yele nɩ nɩbikõo ɩ̃gãn kaafʋ yele. Tɩchɛ a anyãna maa sʋ̃ʋ ba ka ba tʋ̃ɔ nyɔɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ a yelbier vɔlaa pɔ ɛ.
51003001	A lɛ jũu, an ɩ yɩn nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'mataa sɩ̃ɩn a kũu pɔ, yɩ de a yɩ tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a bonsɩ ala na be a saaju, be a Kɩrɩsɩto na jɩ̃nɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nũsʋ̃ɔ jie.
51003002	Yɩ de a yɩ tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a saaju bonsɩ pɔ, tɩ na yɩ ta de a yɩ tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a wɛr ju bonsɩ pɔ ɛ.
51003003	Bojũu yɩ kpi naa, ka a pʋ̃pãanyã ka a yɩ nyɛvʋr sɔɔl a Kɩrɩsɩto a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51003004	An ɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ kʋ yɩ a nyɛvʋr paalaa, 'lɔ wa nyɩr, yɩ mɩ na 'mantãan wʋ nyɩr, na yɩ nyɛ a wʋ tɩɩr.
51003005	A lɛ jũu, yɩ kʋ a ala na be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ na ɩ a wɛr yele. A yelsɩ ala lɛ a anyãna, sɛ̃fʋ yele, dɛɛr yele, vɔldɛɛr, tɩɛr dɛɛr, nɩ bɔgar na nyɛtãan tɩbɛ puorfʋ.
51003006	A bonsɩ anyãna jũu, Nãaŋmɩn suur ire naa.
51003007	A sɔbie anyãna lɛ yɩ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ turo, a lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ.
51003008	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, yɩ tɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin a yelsɩ anyãna pɔ, suur, putuyele, gefʋ, gagar yele, nɩ 'yɛrbidɛbɛ na ma yire a yɩ nɛgãma pɔ.
51003009	Yɩ ta ŋmara jirsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa ɛ. Yɩ ta maala a lɛ go ɛ, yɩ yaa a kõro yele nɩ a wʋ maalfʋsɩ bar,
51003010	tɩ na yɩ su a pʋ̃pãanyã yelpaalaa. Nãaŋmɩn maal yɩn ka yɩ ɩ nɩpaalaa, na wʋ maala yɩ, ka yɩ na kaara a wʋ kaar, ka yɩ na bɔ̃ɔ wʋ yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa.
51003011	Bamɩne ba lɛ chɛnɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ bɩɩ ka bamɩne mɩ ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka bamɩne ŋma yɔɩ bɩɩ ka bamɩne mɩ ba ŋma ɛ, ka bamɩne ɩ sãanba bɩɩ ka bamɩne mɩ ɩ nɩyʋɔrsɩ ɛ, ka bamɩne ɩ gbãgbaar bɩɩ ka bamɩne mɩ ɩ sumɩne ɛ, tɩchɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ ɩ a jaa na wʋ be a jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51003012	A lɛ jũu, an ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kaa ir yɩ, ka yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ na wʋ nʋ̃ yɩ, yɩ pɔɔ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ nɩbaal, vɩla maalfʋ, mɩ̃ɛ siirfʋ, jomm ɩfʋ nɩ kãnyir.
51003013	Yɩ ma tara kãnyir kʋ taa, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa tara nɩ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ 'yɛr, yɩ ma vɛ̃ kʋ taa. Yɩ vɛ̃ bar nɩtãa a lɛ a sɩ Soro na ma vɛ̃ bar yɩ.
51003014	A yelkpɛ̃ɛ jaa lɛ ɩka, yɩ de nʋ̃fʋ su. 'Lɔ lɛ ma nyɔɔ bonsɩ a jaa 'mataa ka a tara nɛbʋ̃'yen.
51003015	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka a Kɩrɩsɩto nyã'maar pire a yɩ nyãn, yɩ jaa pʋɔn a ɩ̃gãn jiir pɔ, na wʋ bʋɔl yɩ ka yɩ tara nyã'maar. Yɩ ma puor wʋ yãan.
51003016	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛrbir di nãa a yɩ pɔ, yɩn wa wile tɩ kpãana taa, nɩ a yɛ̃ wʋ jaa. Yɩ ma yiele Nãaŋmɩn pɛɛfʋ yiel, pʋpɛl yiel, nɩ a yiel na yi a yɩ nyãn pɔ, na yɩ kʋrɔ Nãaŋmɩn.
51003017	Bon 'lɔ jaa yɩn wa maala, ka 'yɛrbir lɛ bɩɩ, ka maalfʋ pɔ lɛ, yɩ ma maal bon jaa, nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor, na yɩ ma tu a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ puor a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn yãan.
51003018	Pɔbɔ, yɩ siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a yɩ sɩrbɛ, lɛ lɛ vɩɛlɛ kʋ a sɩ Soro.
51003019	Sɩrbɛ, yɩ nʋ̃ a yɩ pɔbɔ, na yɩ ta ma pirpire ba ɛ.
51003020	Bibiir, yɩ wõnõ a yɩ dɔɔrbɔ toor yele jaa pɔ, lɛ lɛ pɛlɛ a sɩ Soro pʋɔ.
51003021	Sãamɩne, yɩ ta ma maala ka a yɩ bibiir suur ire ɛ, a lɛ a ba tɩɛr kʋ̃ gã jibʋ̃'yen ɛ.
51003022	Gbãgbaar, yɩ sɔɔrɔ a yɩ nɩbɛrɛ nɛɛ yele jaa pɔ. Yɩ ta ma vɛ̃ ka ba wa fur nɩbir yɔ̃ɔ yɩ, ka yɩ pãa maala a lɛ ban bʋɔrɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ir a yɩ nyãa wʋ jaa 'yɔ̃ɔ, yɩn joro a sɩ Soro dãbɩ̃ɛ jũu.
51003023	Bon jaa yɩn wa maala, yɩ ir a yɩ nyãa 'yɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ ka a kaara fɩka a sɩ Soro lɛ yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ, tɩchɛ a ta ɩ fɩka nɩsaal lɛ yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ ɛ.
51003024	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka yɩn tɩ den a yɩ nãbonsɩ a sɩ Soro sɛ̃ na ɩ a yɩ sãyar. A sɩ Soro Kɩrɩsɩto lɛ yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ.
51003025	Nɩrɛ jaa wa maal yelbier, a yelbier sãyar lɛ wʋn tɩ nyɛ. Nãaŋmɩn ba turo nɩbɛ nʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ.
51004001	Nɩbɛrɛ, yɩ ma kʋrɔ a yɩ gbãgbaar a lɛ na tor na a sɛɛn, bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka yɩ mɩ tara na nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na be a saaju.
51004002	Yɩ de a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ pɔ. Yɩ kaara sʋ̃ na yɩ ma puor wʋ yãan.
51004003	Na yɩ mɩ ma sʋɔrɔ kʋrɔ sɩ ka Nãaŋmɩn na yuo sɔr kʋ a sɩ mʋɔlfʋ ka sɩ na mʋɔl a Kɩrɩsɩto yelsɔɔlsɩ. A 'lɔ pɔ lɛ ba 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ.
51004004	Yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka n na mʋɔl jaa chɛ chɛ chɛ a lɛ an sɛɛn.
51004005	Yɩ ɩ yɛ̃n dẽme nɩ a lɛ yɩn maala a bala na ba ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo sɛ̃. Yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir, yɩn wa nyɛ jie.
51004006	Yɩ ma vɛ̃ ka a yɩ bʋʋr ma ɩ wɩ̃ɛfʋ 'yɛrbie tɩ nʋ̃mɔ̃ nyaar kaar. Ka yɩ na bɔ̃ɔ lɛ yɩn na 'yɛr sɔɔ nɩrɛ 'lɔ wa sʋʋr yɩ 'yɛr.
51004007	Tɩchɩkusɩ na man a maa 'yɛr a jaa kʋ yɩ. Wʋ ɩn a yɛbɛ ɩn nʋ̃ na wʋ mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ. Na wʋ ɩ a tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ sʋɔ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ.
51004008	N tʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ naa a yɩ sɛ̃ ɩka wʋ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a lɛ sɩn ɩrɛ a ka, na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩ nyãn ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
51004009	'Lɔ nɩ Onɩsɩmɔsɩ lɛ 'mataa waara. Wʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ na wʋ ɩ a yɛbɛ sɩn nʋ̃. Wʋ ɩn a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ. Ban man kʋ yɩ bon jaa na ɩrɛ a ka.
51004010	Aristakus mɩ ban 'mataa pɔɔn ma puoro yɩ naa, lɛ lɛ a Maakɩ mɩ na ɩ a Banabasɩ yɛbɛ mɩ puoro yɩ. Yɩ dɔ̃ɔ wõ a wʋ kpãafʋ yele, ala ɩ wʋ wa wan a yɩ sɛ̃, yɩ tuor de wʋ.
51004011	Yesu mɩ ban bʋɔlɔ Jusɩtusɩ mɩ puoro yɩ naa. A nɩbɛ banyãna tɛɛ lɛ ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ pɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ jũu. Ba tara na ɩ̃gãn 'maar kʋ ma.
51004012	Epafaras na ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na wʋ ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃, puoro yɩ naa. Wʋ ma sʋɔrɔ na Nãaŋmɩn nɩbijɩɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ka yɩ na ara kpɛ̃ɔ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ.
51004013	N din a wʋ dãasɩɛ ɩka wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ na kʋrɔ yɩ nɩ a bala na be a Laodisea nɩ a Hɩrapolis tẽn pɔ.
51004014	A sɩ yɛbɛ sɩn nʋ̃, Luka na ɩ a tɩtɩlɛ nɩ Demas puoro yɩ naa.
51004015	Puor Nɩmfa nɩ a pupuorbiir bala na ma tuor a wʋ yir na be a Laodisea.
51004016	Bala wa kar a gãn nyãna kʋ a yɩn Kolose dẽme, yɩ mɔ̃ ka ba mɩ kar wʋ be a Laodisea pupuorbiir pɔ. Yɩ mɔ̃ na yɩ mɩ kar a gãn 'lɔ ɩn sɛb kʋ a Laodisea pupuorbiir.
51004017	'Yɛr kʋ Archipus, "Mɔ̃ tɩ na fʋ baa baar a tʋ̃mɔ̃ ala fʋn nyɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ."
51004018	Maa Pɔɔl lɛ sɛɛrɛ a puorfʋ nyã nɩ a maa mɩ̃ɛ nũu. Yɩ tɩɛr a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ ban 'yɔ̃ɔ ma. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
52001001	Pɔɔl, Silasɩ nɩ Timoti lɛ sɛɛrɛ a gãn nyã kʋrɔ Tɛsalonika pupuorbiir na be a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar wʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃.
52001002	Sɩ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan sɔ̃ɔ jaa kʋ yɩ, tɩ ma tara a yɩ tɩɛr a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ pɔ.
52001003	Sɔ̃ɔ jaa lɛ sɩ ma tɩɛr a yɩ sɔɔfʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃, a yɩ nʋ̃fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ a kãnyir yɩn tara chɛlɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩ a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn.
52001004	Bojũu sɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka, n yɛɛr a yɩn a Nãaŋmɩn na nʋ̃, 'lɔ lɛ kaa ir yɩ.
52001005	Bojũu a sɩ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ na wa a yɩ sɛ̃, ba ɩ 'yɛrbir tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ tara na kpɛ̃ɔ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na ba ɩ baal ɛ. Yɩ mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn a lɛ sɩn be a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn dɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ nɩ yɩ a yɩ jũu.
52001006	Yɩ ɩ naa a sɩn nɩ a Soro tɔtɔɔrbɔ, bojũu dɔɔyɛ kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ lɛ yɩ tu tɩ de a 'yɛrbie nɩ pʋpɛl a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na tɩr,
52001007	lɛ lɛ, yɩn ɩ bʋ̃mansɩ kʋ a bala na sɔɔ de a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ be a Masedonɩya nɩ a Akaya tẽn pɔ.
52001008	Yɩn lɛ yaar a sɩ Soro 'yɛrbie, a ba ɩ a Masedonɩya nɩ a Akaya tẽn pɔ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yaar jie jaa. A lɛ yɩn sɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn yaar jie jaa.
52001009	Ba mɩ̃ɛ lɛ man a lɛ yɩn tuor de sɩ, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn wa a yɩ sɛ̃, nɩ a lɛ yɩn lɩɛb wa a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, tɩ bar a tɩbɛ tɩ wa puoro a nyɛvʋr nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ Nãaŋmɩn,
52001010	tɩ chɛlɛ a wʋ Bie ka wʋ yi saaju wa, a 'lɔ wʋn vɛ̃ ka wʋ lɩɛb ir a kũu pɔ, Yesu a 'lɔ na faa sɩ yɩn a Nãaŋmɩn suur 'lɔ na waara pɔ.
52002001	N yɛɛr, yɩn mɩ̃ɛ jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a yɩ sɛ̃ waa ba ɩ pɔrɔ ɛ,
52002002	sɩn gba na dɔ̃ɔ di dɔɔyɛ a ba ge sɩ be a Filipai tẽe pɔ, nɩtãa yɩn mɩ̃ɛ na bɔ̃ɔn, tɩchɛ sɩ chɛnɛ na tara nyãa a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn pɔ, tɩ man a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ jaa chɛchɛ kʋ yɩ, an sɔɔ ɩ baa sɔɔ de a 'yɛr ɛ.
52002003	Bojũu a sɩ sʋɔrfʋ ba yi jir, bɛlfʋ nɩ tɩɛr dɛɛr pɔ ɛ,
52002004	tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kaa ir sɩ ka sɩ ɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ wiwiilbe. A lɛ jũu lɛ sɩ 'yɛr ɩka, a ba ɩ ka sɩ pɛl nɩsaal pʋɔ ɛ, tɩ sɩ pɛl Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ, a 'lɔ na ma kaara a sɩ pʋtɩɛr.
52002005	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn na ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ɩ a sɩ dãasɩɛ sʋɔ, saa dɔ̃ɔ wa 'yɛr jir 'yɛr bɩɩ ŋmaa jir nyɛ bon ɛ.
52002006	Saa bʋɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩsaal sɛ̃ ɛ, a yɩn mɩ̃ɛ sɛ̃n bɩɩ a sɩ taaba sɛ̃ ɛ, bɩɩ bʋɔrɔ bonsɩ sɩn ɩ Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nsɩ jũu ɛ,
52002007	tɩchɛ sɩ siir a sɩ mɩ̃ɛ a yɩ pɔ, lɛ pɔɔ na ma kaara a wʋ bibiir.
52002008	A lɛ jũu, yɩn kaara sɩ lɛ so ka saa bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ põn yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ tɛɛ ɛ, na sɩ lɔ̃ɔn a sɩ mɩ̃ɛ jaa bojũu a sɩ nʋ̃fʋ ben a yɩ sɛ̃ yɔɔ jaa.
52002009	Sɩrɛ jaa n yɛɛr, yɩ tɩɛr a sɩ kãnyir tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ a dɔɔyɛ. Sɩ tʋ̃n tɩ̃sɔɔ gbulo, nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃gbulo, ka sɩ ta kʋ nɩrɛ jaa tuor ɛ, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋrɔ yɩ ɛ.
52002010	Yɩn lɛ di dãasɩɛ, nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn mɩ na ɩ a Chɛchɛ Sʋɔ nɩ nɩtor tɩ ba tara yele jaa a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a sɩ maalfʋ chaar naa a yɩn na ɩ a sɔɔfʋ dẽme.
52002011	Bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka sɩ ma maal vɩla kʋ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa lɛ sãa na ma maal vɩla kʋ a wʋ bibiir,
52002012	na sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔn yɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn, 'maala yɩ tɩ sʋɔrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩ kpɩɛrɛ a lɛ na pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ, a 'lɔ na bʋɔl yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ tɩɩr pɔ.
52002013	Ala lɛ so ka sɩ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan, bojũu yɩ sɔɔn de a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr yɩn wõ a sɩ sɛ̃, yaa sɔɔ de yaa nɩsaal 'yɛr kaar ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ sɔɔn de yaa Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kaar, ka a tʋ̃nɔ̃ a yɩ bala na sɔɔ de pɔ.
52002014	Bojũu n yɛɛr, yɩn 'lɔ, yɩ ɩ naa tɔtɔɔrbɔ a Nãaŋmɩn puorbo a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ a Judiya, yɩ din dɔɔyɛ a bonsɩ pɔ, a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yelsɩ pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ ban tʋ̃ kʋ a Juu dẽme,
52002015	a bala na kʋ a sɩ Soro Yesu nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ tɩ dii sɩ bar. Ba sɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ tɩ ba sɔɔ nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr ɛ,
52002016	tɩ ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ 'yɛrɛ nɩ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, ka ban nyɛ faafʋ ɛ. Ba kpɛ̃n a yeldɛbɛ pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ kɔkɔɛ. Nãaŋmɩn suur ir naa ka wʋn ge ba.
52002017	Tɩchɛ n yɛɛr, a kor bɩ̃lãa sɩn ba lɛ nyɛ taa ɛ, tɩchɛ saa vɛ̃ a yɩ tɩɛr ɛ. Sɩ mʋ̃ɔn nɩbir ɩka sɩ nyɛ yɩ, na sɩ bʋɔrɔ ɩka a sɩn mɩ̃ɛ sɩ tɩ nyɛ yɩ.
52002018	A la lɛ so ka sɩ ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ wa a yɩ sɛ̃, tɩ maa Pɔɔl ta mʋɔrɔ na bʋɔrɔ, tɩchɛ ka Satan pii a sɩ sɔr.
52002019	Bo lɛ ɩ a sɩ tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie, bɩɩ a pʋpɛl bɩɩ a nyɛvʋr tɩɩr jupil kʋ sɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu waa daar? A ba ɩ yɩn lɛ ɛ?
52002020	Yelmɩ̃ɛ yɩn lɛ ɩ a sɩ tɩɩr nɩ a sɩ pʋpɛl.
52003001	Lɛ an wa gar sɩ a sɩ faa tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a be Atensɩ tẽe pɔ.
52003002	Sɩ tʋ̃n a sɩ yɛbɛ Timoti mɩ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɩ̃sʋɔ na wʋ mʋɔlɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ ɩka wʋ tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ,
52003003	a lɛ ka yɩ taa wa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bɛɛr kaa nyã pɔ ɛ. Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a dɔɔyɛ nyã lɛ sɩn di.
52003004	Yelmɩ̃ɛ, sɩn dɔ̃ɔ be a yɩ sɛ̃, lɛ lɛ sɩ 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka sɩn din dɔɔyɛ. Ka a lɛ mɩ ɩ.
52003005	A lɛ jũu, ɩn kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ lɛ so, ka tʋ̃ nɩrɛ ɩka wʋ tɩ kaa a lɛ a yɩ sɔɔfʋ na be, n dabɩ̃ɛ lɛ ɩka a bɛɛr kaa wʋ taa bɛɛr yɩ kaa, kaa sɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɩ pɔrɔ ɛ.
52003006	Tɩchɛ Timoti yin a yɩ sɛ̃ wa 'yɛr a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ sɩ, a lɛ yɩn tara a sɔɔfʋ nɩ a nʋ̃fʋ. Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ sɩ ɩka yɩ ma tara sɩn nɩ tɩɛr vɩla sɔ̃ɔ jaa na yɩ ma bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ nyɛ sɩ nɩtãa lɛ sɩn mɩ na ma bʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ nyɛ yɩ.
52003007	N yɛɛr, a lɛ jũu, a pʋsɔ̃ɔ nɩ a bɛɛr kaa anyã pɔ, yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩn ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ tun a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ yɩn tara jũu.
52003008	Bojũu pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ pãa na ben be yɩn ara kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ a sɩ Soro.
52003009	Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ sɩn ɩrɛ wa puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan ka a sɛɛ, a pʋpɛl nyã sɩn nyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃?
52003010	Tɩ̃sɔɔ nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ jaa lɛ sɩ ma sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɩka sɩ lɛ nyɛ yɩ go, na sɩ lɛ chɔɔr bon 'lɔ jaa na ba pʋɔ a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ ɛ.
52003011	Pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ sʋɔrɔ naa a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu ɩka, ba yuo sɔr ka sɩ lɛ wa nyɛ yɩ.
52003012	A sɩ Soro wʋ vɛ̃ ka yɩ waa na yɩ nʋ̃nɔ̃ taa, tɩ na yɩ nʋ̃ nɩrɛ jaa nɩtãa lɛ sɩn nʋ̃ yɩ.
52003013	Wʋ vɛ̃ ka yɩ ɩ nɩsʋ̃n na yɩ taa tara dɛɛr jaa a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩ na waan a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ.
52004001	N yɛɛr, a baaraa nɩ nyã, sɩ kpãana yɩ naa a lɛ a yɩ kpɛfʋ na tʋ̃ɔ pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ, nɩtãa lɛ yɩn ben kpɩɛrɛ. Pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa na sɩ kpãkpãana yɩ nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu ɩka yɩ maala a lɛ pʋɔrɔ.
52004002	Bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn wiilfʋ 'lɔ sɩn wiil yɩ tun a sɩ Soro Yesu pɔ.
52004003	A ɩn Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ lɛ wʋn ir yɩ ka yɩ ɩ nɩtorsɩ. A lɛ jũu, yɩ tɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin sɛ̃sɛ̃yele pɔ.
52004004	Ka nɩrɛ jaa tʋ̃ɔ nyɔɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ vɩla, na wʋ ɩ chɛchɛ tɩ tara 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ,
52004005	na yɩ ta bʋɔrɔ pʋpɛl bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ fɩka a nɩbɛ bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ.
52004006	Nɩrɛ jaa wʋ ta maal dɛɛr bɩɩ ŋmɔɔl a wʋ yɛbɛ anyã pɔ ɛ, a sɩ Soro na gen nɩrɛ jaa na maala a anyãna nɩtãa a lɛ sɩn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ yɩ, tɩ na sɩ kpãa yɩ.
52004007	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn ba bʋɔl sɩ ɩka sɩ tara vɔldɛɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ bʋɔrɔ na ɩka sɩ vɛ̃ ka a sɩ kpɛfʋ vɩɛlɛ.
52004008	A lɛ jũu, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na tɔr a wiilfʋ nyã, ba tɔr nɩsaal ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ tɔr a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ na kʋ sɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ.
52004009	A ba lɛ fɛr ɩka, sɩ lɛ sɛb kʋ yɩ a lɛ yɩn na nʋ̃ taa ɛ, bojũu yɩn mɩ̃ɛ jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka, Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa ɩka, yɩ nʋ̃ taa.
52004010	Sɩrɛ jaa yɩ nʋ̃n a yɛɛr na be a Masedonɩya paal pɔ, tɩchɛ sɩ chɛnɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ yɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn ɩka, yɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ sɔ̃ɔ jaa.
52004011	Yɩ vɛ̃ ka a ɩ yɩ nʋ̃ɔ ka a yɩ kpɛfʋ vɩɛlɛ, na yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ tʋ̃mɔ̃ na yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a yɩ nuur nɩtãa a lɛ sɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ.
52004012	Yɩ maal a nɩtɔ̃ ka a yɩ kpɛfʋ na vɩɛlɛ kʋ a bala na ba puor ɛ, na yɩ taa bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩbɛ ba guolo yɩ ɛ.
52004013	N yɛɛr, saa bʋɔrɔ ɩka a lɩɩ yɩ ɛ, nɩ a bala na gur ɛ, na yɩ taa wa tara pʋsɔ̃ɔ fɩka a bala na ba tara tɩɛrtɔ jie kaar ɛ.
52004014	Sɩ sɔɔn ɩka Yesu kpi naa, tɩ na wʋ lɩɛb ir a kũu pɔ. A lɛ lɛ sɩ sɔɔ, ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na 'mantaa waan a Yesu nɩ a bala na gur.
52004015	Sɩ den a sɩ Soro 'yɛrbie 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka, a sɩn bala na chɛnɛ vʋrɔ, tɩ tãn a sɩ Soro waa daar, kʋ̃ dɔ̃ɔ a bala na gur nyɛ wʋ ɛ.
52004016	Bojũu a sɩ Soro mɩ̃ɛ lɛ na yi a saaju wa tãna 'yɛrɛ, ka a malaka kpɛ̃ɛ bʋɔlɔ nɩ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn ɩlɛ pɛɛlɛ ɩrɛ gɔ̃mɔ̃, ka a bala na sɔɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto tɩ kpi, de nie ir.
52004017	A anyã puor, a sɩn bala na chɛnɛ vʋrɔ, a Nãaŋmɩn pãa 'mɔɔr sɩ, ka sɩ lɔ̃ɔtaa tuor a sɩ Soro be julõjuur pɔ, na sɩ tɩ be a wʋ sɛ̃ sɔ̃ɔ jaa.
52004018	A lɛ jũu, yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn naa 'yɛrbie anyãna.
52005001	Pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ n yɛɛr, a ba fɛr ɩka sɩ sɛb bon jaa 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a daar naa sɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
52005002	Bojũu yɩn mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a sɩ Soro Yesu bɩbir na wa naa fɩka nãnyie na ma wa tɩ̃sɔɔ kaar.
52005003	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban wa 'yɛr ɩka, "Nyã'maar ben be, dãbɩ̃ɛ ba lɛ be be ɛ," sɔ̃ɔfʋ na pãa wa naa, a ba sɛ̃, fɩka pɔɔ pʋɔ dɔɔfʋ na dũu wʋ, tɩ ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ faa a ba mɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
52005004	Tɩchɛ yɩn a n yɛɛr, yaa be libe pɔ ɛ, ka a bɩbir nyã na wa dũu yɩ a nãnyie kaar ɛ.
52005005	Yɩ jaa ɩ̃n chãa nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ bibiir, saa ɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ bɩɩ, libe pɔ nɩbɛ ɛ.
52005006	A lɛ jũu, yɩ pãa ta vɛ̃ a sɩ guro nɩbɛ bamɩne kaar ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ vɛ̃ a sɩ jɛɔ na sɩ nyɔɔrɔ sɩ mɩ̃ɛ.
52005007	Bojũu a bala na ma guro, ma gur tɩ̃sɔɔ, ka a bala na buu, mɩ ma buu tɩ̃sɔɔ.
52005008	Tɩchɛ an ɩ a chãa lɛ so sɩ, yɩ vɛ̃ ka sɩ nyɔɔrɔ sɩ mɩ̃ɛ, na sɩ de sɔɔfʋ nɩ nʋ̃fʋ su, fɩka a nyãa wɩɛ nɩ a sɩ tɩɛrtɔfʋ jie na ɩ a sɩ faafʋ kur jupil.
52005009	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn ba ir sɩ ɩka sɩ di dɔɔyɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka sɩ nyɛ faafʋ tu a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
52005010	'Lɔ lɛ kpi kʋ sɩ, a lɛ jũu, ka sɩ chɛnɛ na nɩbir bɩɩ, sɩ gur naa, sɩn nɩ 'lɔ na 'mataa be be.
52005011	A lɛ jũu, yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔn taa ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn na yɩ sʋ̃nɔ̃ taa nɩtãa a lɛ yɩn ben tʋ̃nɔ̃.
52005012	Pʋ̃pãanyã n yɛɛr, sɩ sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa ɩka yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bala na ɩ a yɩ nɩbɛrɛ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a yɩ sɛ̃, bala lɛ sʋ̃nɔ̃ yɩ a sɩ Soro sɔr pɔ, na ba kpãana yɩ.
52005013	Yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba nɩ nʋ̃fʋ a ba tʋ̃mɔ̃ jũu, na yɩ kpɩɛrɛ nɩ nyã'maar nɩ nɩrɛ jaa.
52005014	N yɛɛr n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa ɩka, yɩ kpãana a bala na ɩ a yãan dẽme tɩ na yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bala na sɩɩr a ba mɩ̃ɛ, na yɩ sʋ̃nɔ̃ a nɩbaalsɩ tara kãnyir nɩ nɩrɛ jaa.
52005015	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, ka nɩrɛ jaa ta de yelbier yãan yelbier sãn ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ma maala vɩla kʋrɔ taa nɩ nɩrɛ jaa.
52005016	Yɩ ma tara pʋpɛl sɔ̃ɔ jãa.
52005017	Yɩ ma sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn sɔ̃ɔ jaa.
52005018	Na yɩ ma puor wʋ yãan yele jaa pɔ, bojũu anyã lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
52005019	Yɩ ta kpĩin a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ bũu ɛ.
52005020	Yɩ ta kpɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ wiilfʋ ɛ.
52005021	Yɩ bɛɛr yele jaa kaa na yɩ nyɔɔ bon 'lɔ na vɩla.
52005022	Tɔɔ yi yele jaa na ɩ bier pɔ.
52005023	Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ na ɩ a nyã'maar sʋɔ wʋ chɔɔr yɩ ka yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ. Wʋ maal a yɩ sɩɩr nɩ a yɩ kpɛfʋ nɩ a yɩ ɩ̃gãma ka a ɩ chɛchɛ tɩ ta tara chɛfʋ jaa ɛ, tɩ tãn a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto waa sɔ̃ɔ.
52005024	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã na bʋɔl yɩ tara na yelmɩ̃ɛ, wʋ̃n maal a lɛ.
52005025	N yɛɛr, yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ sɩ.
52005026	Yɩ puor a yɛɛr naa yɛpɔbɔ ba jaa nɩ nʋ̃fʋ puorfʋ.
52005027	N kpãkpãana yɩ naa a sɩ Soro yuor 'yɔ̃ɔ, ɩka yɩ kar a gãn nyã kʋ a yɛɛr ba jaa.
52005028	Ka a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ be a yɩ sɛ̃.
53001001	Pɔɔl, Silasɩ nɩ Timoti lɛ sɛɛrɛ a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a Tɛsalonika pupuorbiir na be a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
53001002	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jie, a be a yɩ sɛ̃.
53001003	N yɛɛr, sɩ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan kʋ yɩ, a mɩ vɩɛl lɛ na a lɛ, bojũu a yɩ sɔɔfʋ nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃, ka a yɩ nʋ̃fʋ yɩn nʋ̃ taa mɩ lɛ nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
53001004	A lɛ jũu, sɩ ma wile na sɩ mɩ̃ɛ pɛɛrɛ yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn pupuorbiir gbulsɩ pɔ, lɛ yɩn tara kãnyir ara kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ a sɔɔfʋ yɩn tara a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ, nɩ a dɔɔyɛ yɩn nyɛrɛ.
53001005	A ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ tor naa, na wʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ maal yɩ ka yɩ sɛɛn a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ, a 'lɔ pɔ yɩn mɩ na dire a dɔɔyɛ.
53001006	Nãaŋmɩn tor naa. Wʋn lɩɛb yab a bala na 'yɛr 'yɛrdɛbɛ, 'yɔ̃ɔ ba gefʋ, tɩ kʋ a bala ban 'yɛr
53001007	'yɛrdɛbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ, pɛ̃nfʋ, nɩ a sɩn mɩ̃ɛ. A nɩtɔ̃ na ɩ naa, Nãaŋmɩn na wa ir a sɩ Soro Yesu wiil a saaju nɩ a wʋ kpɩ̃ɛn malakasɩ, fɩka bũu dagel.
53001008	Wʋn gen a bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, na baa sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro Yesu 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ ɛ.
53001009	Bala lɛ na nyɛ gefʋ 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. Wʋn oor ban yɩn a sɩ Soro niem, nɩ a wʋ tɩɩr kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ.
53001010	'Lɔ wa wa a bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, wʋn nyɛn 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ pɔ. An ɩn nʋ̃ɔ kʋ a bala jaa na sɔɔ de wʋ. Yɩ mɩ pʋɔ naa, bojũu yɩ sɔɔn de a sɩ dãasɩɛ sɩn di a yɩ sɛ̃.
53001011	A anyã tɩɛr sɩn tara jũu, sɩ ma sʋɔrɔ na Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka wʋ vɛ̃ ka yɩ sɛɛn a wʋ bʋɔlfʋ, ka a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka a yi tɩɛr vɩɛlsɩ nɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ jaa na yi a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ.
53001012	A anyãna lɛ sɩ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn ɩka a sɩ Soro Yesu yuor wʋ nyɛ tɩɩr a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka wʋ mɩ pɛɛ yɩ, a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu.
53002001	A lɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto waa sɔ̃ɔ nɩ a lɛ sɩn na lɔ̃ɔ taa a wʋ sɛ̃, sɩ sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa, n yɛɛr,
53002002	ɩka yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a sɔb yɩ nɩbir a nɩbɛ bamɩne na 'yɛrɛ ɩka sɩn lɛ 'yɛr bɩɩ, sɛb ɩka a Yesu wan baar.
53002003	Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa bɛl yɩ a sɔr nyã pɔ ɛ, a bɩbir 'lɔ kʋ̃ wa ɛ, ka a bawõnsɩ ba de nie ir ɛ. Ka a 'lɔ na ba sɔɔ de a nɛbinãa mɩ yi chãa pɔ, 'lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na sɔ̃ɔ.
53002004	Wʋ ma chɩrɛ naa tɩ na wʋ ma 'mɔɔrɔ, wʋ mɩ̃ɛ gar Nãaŋmɩn, bɩɩ bon jaa ban puoro, a lɛ lɛ wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir maal a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn.
53002005	Yaa lɩɛb tɩɛr ɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a bonsɩ anyãna a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn be a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ?
53002006	Pʋ̃pãanyã yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa a bon 'lɔ na pii wʋ a sɔr a wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ yɩ chãa pɔ ɛ, a wʋ sɔ̃ɔ baa wa ta ɛ.
53002007	A wʋ yelsɔɔlaa tʋ̃nɔ̃ na tʋ̃mɔ̃, tɩchɛ a 'lɔ na pii a sɔr yi be.
53002008	Ka a bala na ba sɔɔ de a nɛbinãa ɛ na yin chãa pɔ, a bala a Soro Yesu nɩ naa sɔ̃ɔn a wʋ nɛɛ vʋʋr, sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yele 'lɔ na ɩrɛ a wʋ waa sɔ̃ɔ.
53002009	A bala na ba sɔɔ de a nɛbinãa ɛ, na wa naa an ɩ a Satan tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ, a 'lɔ na de kpɛ̃ɔ, jɩ̃nsɩ nɩ jire, nɛ'maa yelsɩ,
53002010	nɩ yelbier jaa bʋrɔ bɛlfʋ sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a nɩbɛ bala na wɛrɛ, ba wɛrɛ naa, bojũu ba tɔr naa ɩka ba nʋ̃ a yelmɩ̃ɛ na ba nyɛ faafʋ.
53002011	A lɛ jũu, Nãaŋmɩn na sɔɔ naa ka yele kɔ̃ɔ bɛl ba, nɩ lɛ ban sɔɔ de bon 'lɔ na ɩ jire.
53002012	A lɛ jũu, bala jaa na ba sɔɔ de a yelmɩ̃ɛ a ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa jũu, nɩ a bon 'lɔ na ba tor ɛ, na nyɛn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ.
53002013	Tɩchɛ sɩn 'lɔ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan kʋrɔ yɩ, n yɛɛr, a yɩn a sɩ Soro na nʋ̃, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn kãan ir yɩ a pielfʋ daar ka yɩn nyɛ faafʋ, ka a wʋ Sɩɛ pɛɛrɛ yɩ a yɩ sɔɔ de a yelmɩ̃ɛ.
53002014	'Lɔ lɛ bʋɔl yɩ a anyãna pɔ, a lɛ yɩn wõ sɩn mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ yɩ. Lɛ lɛ ka yɩn lɔ̃ɔ põn a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tɩɩr.
53002015	A lɛ jũu, n yɛɛr yɩ ara kpɛ̃ɔ na yɩ nyɔɔ a sɩ wiilfʋ sɩn wiil yɩ, ka 'yɛrbir lɛ bɩɩ, nɛɛ lɛ bɩɩ, gãn pɔ lɛ.
53002016	A sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ̃ɛ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a sɩ Sãa na nʋ̃ sɩ tun a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ pɔ, na 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩn ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, nɩ tɩɛrtɔ vɩla,
53002017	wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn a yɩ nyãa pɔ nɩ vɩla jaa nɩ a 'yɛrbie pɔ.
53003001	N yɛɛr, a baarfʋ nɩ nyã, yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ sɩ, ka a sɩ Soro 'yɛrbie tʋ̃ɔ yaar fɔɔ tɩ nyɛ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ jie jaa nɩtãa lɛ an be a yɩ pɔ.
53003002	Na yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn ka sɩ na tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ faafʋ yin a putudẽme nɩ a sɩdɛbɛ dẽme nuur pɔ, bojũu nɩrɛ jaa baa tara a sɔɔfʋ ɛ.
53003003	Tɩchɛ a sɩ Soro ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩn ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ tɩ gu yɩ a dɛɛr sʋɔ nuur pɔ.
53003004	Sɩ tara na sɔɔfʋ a sɩ Soro yuor 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩ pɔ ɩka, yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ na, na yɩn chɛnɛ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a ala sɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ.
53003005	A sɩ Soro wʋ vɛ̃ a yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃ yɩ naa nɩ lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na tara nɩ yɩ a kãnyir.
53003006	A sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor pɔ, sɩ kpãana yɩ naa n yɛɛr ɩka yɩ tɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin a bala na ɩ koro dẽme pɔ, nɩ ban ba turo a lɛ sɩn wiil yɩ ɩka yɩ turo ɛ.
53003007	Yɩn mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a sɛɛ naa ɩka yɩ tɔɔrɔ sɩ, saa dɔ̃ɔ yʋɔrɔ pɔrɔ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn be a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ,
53003008	bɩɩ saa dɔ̃ɔ di nɩrɛ jaa bʋ̃diir tɩ na saa yab ɛ. Sɩ ma tʋ̃n tʋ̃kpɩ̃ɛn tɩ̃sɔɔ nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ, ka sɩ ta tuo a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tuor ɛ.
53003009	A nyã ba wiil ɩka saa tara sɔr na ɩ a lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ kaa ɩ wiilfʋ kʋ yɩ ka yɩ tɔɔrɔ.
53003010	Sɩ gba na dɔ̃ɔ be a yɩ sɛ̃, sɩ kpãkpãan yɩ naa a yele nyãna ɩka, nɩrɛ jaa ba wa tʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, wʋ taa dire ɛ.
53003011	Sɩ wõn ban 'yɛr ɩka nɩbɛ bamɩne ben a yɩ pɔ tara koro na ba yʋɔrɔ pɔrɔ, na baa tara tʋ̃mɔ̃ jaa ɛ, tɩ ma kpɩɛrɛ a ba taaba yelsɩ pɔ.
53003012	A nɩbɛ banyãna taa ba, sɩ 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor pɔ ɩka, ba tʋ̃ a ba tʋ̃mɔ̃ jaa jomm na ba nyɛ a ba mɩ̃ɛ bonsɩ.
53003013	N yɛɛr, yɩn 'lɔ yɩ taa wa bal nɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ 'lɔ na tor pɔ ɛ.
53003014	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ ba wa sɔɔ de a lɛ sɩn 'yɛr a gãn nyã pɔ ɛ, yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wʋ yele sʋ̃ na yɩ taa tara nɩ wʋ nɛbʋ̃'yen ɛ, ka vɩ̃ kpɛ wʋ.
53003015	Yɩ ta de wʋ ka wʋ ɩ dɔ̃sʋɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ kpãa wʋ wʋn ɩ a yɩ wʋn ɩ a yɛbɛ jũu.
53003016	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a sɩ Soro na ɩ nyã'maar sʋɔ wʋ kʋ yɩ nyã'maar sɔ̃ɔ jaa, a sɔɩ a jaa pɔ. A sɩ Soro wʋ be a yɩ jaa sɛ̃.
53003017	Maa Pɔɔl lɛ sɛb a puorfʋ nyã nɩ a maa mɩ̃ɛ nũu. A jɩ̃nɛ naa nyã ɩn ma 'yɔ̃ɔ gãn jaa pɔ ɩn ma sɛb.
53003018	A sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ a be a yɩ jaa sɛ̃.
54001001	Maa Pɔɔl na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nãa, nɩtãa lɛ a sɩ Fafaara Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛr nɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ tɩɛrtɔ jie.
54001002	N sɛɛrɛ na kʋrɔ a Timoti na ɩ a n binʋ̃nãa sɔɔfʋ jũu. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ, nɩ nɩbaal, nɩ nyã'maar na yi a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃, a be a fʋ sɛ̃.
54001003	A lɛ ɩn chen a Masedonɩya, n kpãkpãan fʋ naa ɩka fʋ jɩ̃nɛ a Efesus na fʋ wile a nɩbɛ bamɩne a ba taa wile wiil yuo go ɛ.
54001004	Wiilfʋ ba ka ba ta de ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ jir wiilfʋ ɛ, nɩ a sãakpãmɩne tutaa na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. A anyãna lɛ waara nɩ nɛchɩrɛ, ban naa tʋ̃nɔ̃ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ nɩ sɔɔfʋ.
54001005	Tɩchɛ a wiilfʋ nyã lɛ waara nɩ nʋ̃fʋ na yi nyãvɩla pɔ, tɩɛr vɩla pɔ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔɔfʋ pɔ.
54001006	Nɩbɛ bamɩne bar naa a anyã tɩ na ba 'yɛrɛ 'yɛr vorsɩ.
54001007	Ba bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba ɩ a nɛɛ wiwiilbe, na baa bɔ̃ɔ a par a lɛ ban 'yɛrɛ ɛ, bɩɩ na a bonsɩ ala ban 'yɛr ɩka a sɛɛ naa ɛ.
54001008	Faa nyɛ, sɩn bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a nɛbinãa vɩla na, ala ɩ nɩrɛ tun a lɛ an wile.
54001009	Sɩ mɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka, a nɛbinãa ba bin kʋ a nɩtorsɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ bin kʋ a bala na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nɛɛ, nɩ a bawõnsɩ, nɩ a bala na ba turo lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔr ɛ, yelbe-ɩrbɛ, nɩ a bala na ba puoro ɛ, na ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn yuor, nɩ a bala na kʋrɔ a ba sãamɩne, nɩ a ba mamɩne na ba ɩ nɩkʋrbɔ,
54001010	nɩ a sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ, nɩ a bala na lɩɛb bʋɔr taa, nɩ a bala na lɩɛb daara a ba taaba, nɩ a jir ŋmarba, nɩ a bala na ŋmara jir pɔrɔ nɩ, nɩ yele jaa na chɩrɛ nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ wiilfʋ.
54001011	A wiilfʋ anyã yire na a dãnfʋ Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a tɩɩr sʋɔ 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ wʋn de kʋ ma sɛ̃.
54001012	N puor naa a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yãan, wʋn kʋ ma kpɛ̃ɔ bojũu wʋ nyɛn a n sɔɔfʋ, na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ.
54001013	N gba na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn yosɔ̃ɔnɔ̃, gere a nɩbɛ, naa ɩ jɛbʋɔrɔ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn wa kãan a n nɩbaal, bojũu n ɩn a lɛ ɩn ba sɔɔ de nɩ babɔ̃ɔfʋ jũu,
54001014	tɩchɛ a sɩ Soro wɩ̃ɛfʋ waa naa, nɩ a sɔɔfʋ, nɩ a nʋ̃fʋ ala na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
54001015	A yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr nɩ nyã, na a ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ sɔɔ de. Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wan a wɛr pɔ ɩka wʋ wa faa yelbe-ɩrbɛ, tɩchɛ maa lɛ gar ba jaa.
54001016	Tɩchɛ a lɛ jũu lɛ so ka Nãaŋmɩn kaa n nɩbaal, ka a na tʋ a n pɔ, a maa na ɩ a yelbe-ɩrɛ gar ba jaa, ka Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wiil a wʋ kãnyir na ba tara baarfʋ kʋ ma, ka n ɩ wiilfʋ kʋ a bala na wa sɔɔ wʋ nyɛ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baar fʋ ɛ.
54001017	Pʋ̃pãanyã a Nãa 'lɔ na ba tara pielfʋ ɛ, a 'lɔ na ba kpire ɛ, a 'lɔ sɩn ba nyɛrɛ ɛ, a Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ, wʋ nyɛrɛ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ tɩɩr bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
54001018	N bie Timoti, n kʋrɔ fʋ naa a wiilfʋ anyãna tun a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a fʋ 'yɛr, ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ turo a lɛ, fʋn jɛb a jɛb vɩla 'lɔ.
54001019	Tara sɔɔfʋ nɩ pʋtɩvɩla, bojũu nɩbɛ bamɩne tɔr naa a vɩla 'lɔ maalfʋ bar ka a ba sɔɔfʋ bʋ̃bʋr.
54001020	A ba pɔ lɛ Hɩmɩnayas nɩ Aleksanda, bala lɛ n de kʋ a Satan ka ba na jãn ta fere sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn yuor ɛ.
54002001	A lɛ jũu, a ala na de nie nɩ nyã, n kpãkpãan yɩn ɩka yɩ sʋɔrɔ, Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ, na yɩ ma sʋɔrɔ kʋrɔ taa, tɩ na yɩ ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan kʋ nɩrɛ jaa.
54002002	Yɩ mɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ a nãmɩne nɩ a bala na ɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, ka a lɛ na vɛ̃ ka sɩn jɛ̃n ɩ̃gãn 'maar nɩ nyã'maar na sɩ maala a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ.
54002003	A nyã lɛ tor, naa pɛlɛ a sɩ Fafaara Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ.
54002004	'Lɔ lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩrɛ jaa wʋ nyɛ faafʋ, na wʋ wa bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ.
54002005	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ be be, nɩ 'ma'maala bʋ̃'yen na be a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a nɩsaalba chara pɔ, 'lɔ lɛ a nɩrɛ Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto.
54002006	'Lɔ lɛ de a wʋ nyɛvʋr yab faan nɩrɛ jaa. A 'yɛr nyã lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ sɩ ɩka sɩ mʋɔl a pʋ̃pãanyã.
54002007	A lɛ lɛ so ka Nãaŋmɩn ir ma ka ɩ mʋmʋɔlɔ nɩ a nɩtʋ̃nãa. Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ n 'yɛrɛ, n ba ŋmara jir ɛ, ɩka n ɩ a wiwile kʋ a bala na ba ɩ a Juu nɩbɛ ɛ, sɔɔfʋ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ pɔ.
54002008	Maa bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka jie jaa, a dɔɔr wa sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn, ba jɛɛr a ba nuur puoro, na ba maala a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ, na ba ta tara suur nɩ nɛchɩrɛ ɛ.
54002009	Lɛ lɛ a pɔbɔ mɩ, ba ma su bon pɔɔ a ɩ̃gãn, tɩ na ba ta ma mal pir a jukɔɔl nɩ a sɛlma nɩ a lɛrsɩ bɩɩ a fɔɔr ala daa na ɩ tuo ɛ,
54002010	tɩchɛ tʋ̃sʋ̃n lɛ sɛɛn a pɔbɔ bala na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn.
54002011	Pɔbɔ ba ma jãn ɩ gbul na ba siir ba mɩ̃ɛ chɛlɛ a lɛ a nɩdierbe na wile.
54002012	N ba bar sɔr ɩka pɔɔ jaa wʋ wile bɩɩ tara kpɛ̃ɔ daba ju ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ma ɩ gbul.
54002013	Bojũu Adama lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn de nie mɛ tɩ na wʋ wa mɛ a Hawa tu.
54002014	Satan ba dɔ̃ɔ nie bɛl Adama ɛ, tɩchɛ a Hawa lɛ wʋ bɛl ka wʋ sɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ.
54002015	Tɩchɛ a pɔbɔ na nyɛn faafʋ tu bie dɔɔfʋ pɔ, ala ɩ ba chɛnɛ na tara sɔɔfʋ nɩ nʋ̃fʋ na ba ɩ chɛchɛ nyɔɔrɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ vɩla.
54003001	A 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ a pupuorbiir nɩdiere, wʋ bʋɔrɔ na tʋ̃sʋ̃.
54003002	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a pupuorbiir nɩdiere wʋ ta tara mabfʋ jaa ɛ, na wʋ tara pɔɔ bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ, na wʋ nyɔɔrɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, na wʋ ɩ nɩ'yɔ̃ɔ naa, na wʋ diere sãanba, na wʋ bɔ̃ɔ wiilfʋ.
54003003	Wʋ ta ɩ dãburo ɛ, wʋ ta ɩ gɔ̃bʋɔr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ siir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, na wʋ ta ɩ jɛbʋɔrɔ ɛ, na wʋ ta nʋ̃ libie ɛ.
54003004	A sɛɛn ɩka wʋ tʋ̃ɔ kaara a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yir vɩla, ka a wʋ bibiir wõnõ a wʋ toor, na ba 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ wʋ.
54003005	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yir kaa ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ wʋn ɩ tʋ̃ɔ kaa a pupuorbiir?
54003006	Wʋ ta ɩ nɩrɛ nyã na kpɛ a puorfʋ pɔ paal ɛ, na wʋn wa bʋɔrɔ yuor na wʋ mɩ faa lo a gefʋ pɔ nɩtãa a Satan.
54003007	Wʋ ɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ a bala na ba puoro ɛ, na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃, ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, ban 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋn vɩ̃ ka wʋ lo a Satan bɛraa pɔ.
54003008	A sʋ̃sʋ̃nbɔ, ba mɩ tara nɩbijɩɛ na ba ta tara nɛɛr ayi ɛ, na ba ta maal ba mɩ̃ɛ dãnyurbo ɛ, na ba ta ɩ nɩfɔlbɔ ɛ.
54003009	Ba nyɔɔ a sɔɔfʋ wiilfʋ yelsɔɔlaa kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ tɩɛr vɩla.
54003010	Yɩ de nie bɛɛr ba kaa. Ka bala pãa baa tara 'mabfʋ jaa ɛ, yɩ vɛ̃ ka ba ɩ a sʋ̃sʋ̃nbɔ.
54003011	A pɔbɔ mɩ, ba tara 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, na ba ta sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa yoe ɛ, tɩchɛ ba nyɔɔrɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ, tɩ tara yelmɩ̃ɛ yele jaa pɔ.
54003012	A sʋ̃sʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ tara pɔɔ bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ, na wʋ tʋ̃ɔ kaara a wʋ bibiir, na wʋ tʋ̃ɔ kaara a wʋ yir vɩla.
54003013	A sʋ̃sʋ̃nbɔ bala na tʋ̃ vɩla, na nyɛn 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋ a ba mɩ̃ɛ, nɩ a 'lafʋ nɩ sɔɔfʋ 'lɔ ban tara a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ.
54003014	N bʋɔrɔ na ɩka n wa a fʋ sɛ̃ a pʋ̃pãanyã, tɩchɛ n sɛɛrɛ na a kpãafʋ anyã kʋrɔ fʋ.
54003015	Lɛ lɛ, maa baa tʋ̃ɔ wa fɔɔ ɛ, ka fʋ bɔ̃ɔ lɛ an sɛɛ ɩka a pupuorbiir ba nyɔɔrɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ, bala lɛ puoro a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ vʋr na ba tɩɛ a yelmɩ̃ɛ a luur kaar.
54003016	Baal ba be be ɛ, a yelsɔɔlaa a sɩ puorfʋ pɔ bɛrma naa. Yesu nyɩr a ɩ̃gãn pɔ. Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ir wiil ɩka wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn bie. A malakasɩ nyɛ wʋ naa. Ba mʋɔl 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr a paalsɩ pɔ, ka ba sɔɔ de wʋ a wɛr wʋ jaa. Nãaŋmɩn de wʋn don be a tɩɩr pɔ.
54004001	Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr ka a gã chãa pɔ ɩka a baaraa, bamɩne na bar a ba sɔɔfʋ tɩ chɛlɛ a sɩdɛbɛ bɛlfʋ, nɩ a lɛ a sɩdɛbɛ na wile.
54004002	A wiilfʋ nyã yi naa a nɛɛr ayi dẽme na ma ŋmara a jirsɩ ka a sɔ̃ɔ a ba tɩɛr fɩka kur tʋl ban 'mon bon 'yɔ̃ɔ jɩ̃nɛ.
54004003	Ba wile na nɩbɛ ɩka ba ta kultaar ɛ, na ba wile ba ɩka ba chire bʋ̃diir amɩne. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn na maal a kultaa nɩ a bʋ̃diir a jaa ɩka a bala na sɔɔ tɩ bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ, ba ma de tɩ puor wʋ yãan.
54004004	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃maalaa jaa vɩɛlɛ na, ka a ba sɛɛ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ tɔr bon jaa bar ɛ, ala ɩ sɩ ma den nɩ yãan puorfʋ.
54004005	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbir nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ maal yaa naa ka a ɩ bʋ̃sʋ̃.
54004006	Ala ɩ fʋ den a kpãafʋ nyã na fʋ wiil a yɛɛr, fʋn ɩn a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tʋ̃tʋ̃vɩla sʋɔ, na fʋn guolo a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nɩ a sɔɔfʋ wiil vɩla 'lɔ fʋn turo.
54004007	Tɔr a jirsɩ ala ban ma ŋmara nɩ a pɔɔnyɔ̃n fuolsɩ, tɩ na fʋ wile a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn sɔr pɔ.
54004008	Bojũu fʋ̃ʋ jãn a fʋ ɩ̃gãn ka wʋ kpɛ̃mɛ, a vɩla na, tɩ wʋ kʋ̃ kor ɛ, tɩchɛ a Nãaŋmɩn sɔr tufʋ vɩla na a sɔɩ a jaa pɔ, bojũu wʋ tɩr nɛɛ kʋ sɩ a nyɛvʋr nyã sɩn tara a dɩna nɩ a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na waara daar kɔ̃ɔ.
54004009	A 'yɛr nyã ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka, nɩrɛ jaa wʋ sɔɔ de.
54004010	A lɛ jũu lɛ sɩ mʋɔrɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ tʋ̃kpɩ̃ɛn, bojũu a sɩ tɩɛrtɔ ben a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ vʋr pɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ a nɩbɛ bala jaa na sɔɔ wʋ Fafaara.
54004011	Kpãkpãana na fʋ wile ba a yelsɩ anyãna a jaa.
54004012	Ta vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa kaa fʋ pɔrɔ fʋn chɛnɛ ɩ pɔlbile jũu ɛ, tɩchɛ fʋ ɩ wiilfʋ kʋ a bala na tara sɔɔfʋ, nɩ a fʋ 'yɛr, nɩ a fʋ maalfʋ, nɩ a fʋ nʋ̃fʋ, nɩ a fʋ sɔɔfʋ, nɩ a fʋ chɛchɛ ɩfʋ pɔ.
54004013	Sɛrɛ tɩchɛ ka n wa, mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir kara a Nãaŋmɩn gãn a nɩyɔɔ pɔ, na fʋ mʋɔlɔ tɩ wile nɩ ba.
54004014	Ta mel a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn kʋ fʋ ɛ, a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a nɩdierbe na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr tɩ dɔɔl fʋ a ba nuur.
54004015	De a yelsɩ a nyã tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃, na fʋ de fʋ mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ, ka nɩrɛ jaa nyɛ lɛ a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ na chiine niem.
54004016	Bɔ̃ɔ nyɔɔ a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a wiilfʋ ɩrɛ a lɛ nɛ, na fʋ tara kãnyir. Fʋn faan a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩ a bala na chɛlɛ a fʋ 'yɛr.
54005001	Ta 'yɛr 'yɛrbikpɩ̃ɛn kʋ danyɔ̃n ɛ, tɩchɛ 'yɛr baalʋ̃ʋ kʋ wʋ fʋ sãa tɔ sʋɔ kaar, 'yɛr kʋ pɔlbil a fʋ yɛɛr kaar.
54005002	'Yɛrɛ nɩ a pɔɔnyɔ̃n a fʋ mamɩne kaar, nɩ a pɔɔsarbil a fʋ yɛpɔbɔ kaar, nɩ chɛchɛ ɩfʋ pɔ.
54005003	'Yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a pɔɔkɔɛ bala na ɩ pɔɔkɔɛ, tɩ ba tara bon jaa ɛ.
54005004	Ala ɩ a pɔɔkɔnyɩnɛ tara na bibiir bɩɩ yɔ̃n, bala lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka ba turo a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ, na ba kaara a ba dɔɔrbɔ a yie pɔ fɩka a lɛ a ba dɔɔrbɔ na dɔ̃ɔ kaa ba. Lɛ lɛ pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ.
54005005	Pɔɔkʋɔr 'lɔ na ba tara bon jaa ɛ, ma den a wʋ tɩɛr wʋ jaa kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, tɩ na wʋ ma sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn tɩ̃sɔɔ nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ a wʋ bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ,
54005006	tɩchɛ a pɔɔkʋɔr 'lɔ na bʋɔrɔ ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa, wʋ kpin tɩ yʋɔrɔ.
54005007	Kʋ ba a kpãafʋ anyãna, ka nɩrɛ ta nyɛ a ba 'mabfʋ ɛ.
54005008	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ baa sʋ̃ʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ ɛ, bɩɩ a wʋ yir dẽme ɛ, a kaara fɩka wʋ tɔr naa a sɔɔfʋ, tɩ ɩrɛ dɛɛr gar nyã na ba ɩ a Yesu turo ɛ.
54005009	A pɔɔkʋɔr 'lɔ na ba ta yuom lɩjaata sɛrɛ ɛ, taa ɩrɛ wa 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wʋ yuor a pɔɔkɔɛ gãn pɔ ɛ. Wʋ ɩ pɔɔkʋɔr 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ kul sɩr bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ, ka a sɩrɛ wa kpi tɩ chɛ wʋ bar, tɩ wʋ chɛnɛ nyɔɔrɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ba kul sɩrɛ go ɛ.
54005010	Nɩbɛ ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ a wʋ tʋ̃ vɩla jũu, nɩ a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ guol a wʋ bibiir, na wʋ ma sɔɔ diere sãanba, na wʋ ma pɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ gbɛɛ, sʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a nɩbaalsɩ, tɩ maala vɩla jaa bʋrɔ.
54005011	Tɩchɛ ta 'yɔ̃ɔ pɔɔkɔ'yɔlɔ yuor a pɔɔkɔɛ gãn pɔ ɛ, bojũu sɩrɛ kulfʋ vɔlaa wa gar a lɛ ban nʋ̃ a Kɩrɩsɩto, ban bʋɔrɔ na sɩrɛ kulfʋ.
54005012	A lɛ ban lon Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ pɔ, bojũu ba sɔ̃ɔn a nɛɛ ban põl'yɔ̃ɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto bar.
54005013	A lɛ puor, ba ma bʋɔrɔ na ɩka ba yʋɔrɔ pɔrɔ tulo yie yʋɔrɔ, a ba ɩ yie tuulfʋ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩ ba ɩn gagarsɩ, na ba kpɩɛrɛ nɩbɛ 'yɛr 'yɛrsɩ pɔ 'yɛrɛ a lɛ na ba sɛɛ ɩka ba 'yɛrɛ ɛ.
54005014	A lɛ jũu, n bʋɔrɔ na ɩka pɔɔkɔɛ na chɛnɛ kpɩ̃ɛn, ba kul sɩrbɛ, na ba dɔɔ bibiir, na ba tʋ̃ɔ ɩ pɔɔ mɩn kaara a ba yie, na ba ta kʋ a dɔ̃sʋɔ sɔr ka wʋ sɔ̃ɔ a sɩ yuor ɛ.
54005015	Bamɩne lɩɛb sɩrɛ jaa turo a Satan puor.
54005016	Ala ɩ pɔɔ nyã jaa na puoro tara yir dẽme ka ba ɩ pɔɔkɔɛ, wʋ kaara ba tɩ ta kʋ a pupuorbiir wõm ɛ. A pupuorbiir ba kaara pɔɔkɔɛ bala tɛɛ na ba tara nɩrɛ jaa, ka wʋn kaa ba ɛ.
54005017	A nɩdierbe bala na tʋ̃nɔ̃ vɩla, yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba, tɩ sʋ̃nɔ̃ ba nɩ bonsɩ, bala lɛ mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr tɩ wile.
54005018	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn gãn 'yɛr ɩka, "Ta lũ a nadar nɛɛ 'lɔ wa vara a chi ɛ." A tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ jaa sɛɛn na a wʋ sãyar.
54005019	Taa ɩrɛ wa sɔɔrɔ nɩbʋ̃'yen 'yɛr wʋn 'yɛr dɔɔl a nɩdiere ju ka bala ba ta ayi bɩɩ ata ɛ.
54005020	A bala na ma maala a yeldɛbɛ, wiil ba a ba sɔ̃ɔnaa a nɩyɔɔ niem, ka a ba taaba na chɛ na joro dãbɩ̃ɛ.
54005021	N kpãana yɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩ a malakasɩ bala wʋn ir niem ɩka, yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a kpãafʋ anyãna pɔ, na yɩ ta oor ɛ. Yɩ taa turo nɩbɛ nʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ.
54005022	Ta pɔɔ ir nɩrɛ ka wʋ ɩ nɩdiere ɛ, ta pʋɔ a nɩbɛ bamɩne yeldɛbɛ pɔ ɛ, gu fʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
54005023	Ta nyuro kʋ̃ɔ tɛɛ ɛ, ma nyũ dãa bɩ̃lãa a fʋ pʋɔ baal jũu, a fʋn maa yaar tɩ ɩ baal ɛ.
54005024	Nɩbɛ bamɩne yeldɛbɛ gãn chãa pɔ, na a dɔ̃ɔ ba nie chen a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie, tɩchɛ ka bamɩne yeldɛbɛ ma tu ba chen a be.
54005025	Lɛ lɛ a tʋ̃vɩɛl amɩne ma gãn chãa pɔ, a ala gba na ba yi ɛ, kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɔɔl ɛ.
54006001	Bala jaa na be a gbãgbaar tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ, ba 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a bala na tʋ̃ɔ ba, ka nɩrɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn yuor 'yɛrdɛɛr ɛ, nɩ a sɩ wiilfʋ ɛ.
54006002	A gbãgbaar bala na tara a nɩbɛrɛ a ba ɩ Yesu turbo, ba ta vɛ̃ ba 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ ɛ, ban 'mataa puoro jũu ɛ, ba ir nyãa 'yɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ ba, bojũu ba puoro naa ka ba nʋ̃ ba. Wile a anyãna na fʋ kpãkpãana ba.
54006003	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ wiil wiil yor na ba tu a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wiilfʋ ɛ, nɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbie na 'yɛr ɛ,
54006004	a nɩbɛ nyã wile na wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, na waa bɔ̃ɔ bon jaa ɛ. Wʋ ma chɩrɛ na nɩ a 'yɛrbie, bojũu a nyɛntãan fɩka a wʋ tɩɛr sɔ̃ɔ naa. A lɛ vɛ̃ naa ka wʋ tara nyuur na wʋ ma jɛɛrɛ, na wʋ ma tʋrɔ a wʋ taaba, na wʋ ma tara tɩɛr dɛɛr nɩ a wʋ taaba.
54006005	Na ba pãa ma chɩrɛ taa nɩ tɩɛr sɔ̃ɔnsɩ. Baa bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, na ba tɩɛr ɩka a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ ɩn lefʋ yele lɛ.
54006006	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn sɔr tufʋ ɩn lefʋ bon, ala ɩ a ala fʋn tara sɛɛn fʋ naa.
54006007	Bojũu saa waan bon jaa a wɛr nyã pɔ ɛ, na sɩ kʋ̃ lɛ de bon jaa yin a wɛr pɔ ɛ.
54006008	A lɛ jũu, ala ɩ sɩ tara na bʋ̃diir nɩ bʋ̃sursɩ, sɩ vɛ̃ ka a sɛɛn sɩ.
54006009	A bala na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba ɩ tara dẽme, ma lon bɛɛr kaa chɛbaa pɔ, ka jɔl tɩɛr nɩ vɔldɛbɛ ma tɔɔ a nɩbɛ chiine sɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ a wɛfʋ jie.
54006010	Bojũu libie nʋ̃fʋ ɩ naa yelbier jaa bʋrɔ nyɩɩr, ka a bamɩne na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba le, ba tɔɔn jãan a yelmɩ̃ɛ, na ba kpɛ wõm pɔ.
54006011	Tɩchɛ a fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩrɛ, tɔɔ yi a anyãna a jaa pɔ, na fʋ turo yeltorsɩ, na fʋ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩrɛ, tara sɔɔfʋ na fʋ tara nʋ̃fʋ, na fʋ tara kãnyir, na fʋ ɩ nɩ hɛ lɛ lɛ lɛ.
54006012	Jɛb a sɔɔfʋ jɛɛr na fʋ nyɔɔ a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ taa lɛɛ. 'Lɔ pɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl fʋ a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ fʋn chiir a fʋ pʋɔ a nɩyɔɔ niem.
54006013	N kpãkpãana fʋ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na kʋrɔ a bonsɩ a jaa nyɛvʋr niem, nɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na 'yɛr a wʋ yelmɩ̃ɛ na wʋ chiir a wʋ pʋɔ a nãa Pontius Pilate niem,
54006014	n kpãkpãana fʋ naa ɩka fʋ bɔ̃ɔ tara a Nãaŋmɩn nɛbinsɩ ka a ta tara dɛɛr, bɩɩ 'mabfʋ ɛ, tɩ tãn a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto waa daar.
54006015	'Lɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na waan a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ. Nãaŋmɩn tɛɛ lɛ sɛɛn dãnfʋ nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ, na wʋ ɩ a nãmɩne ba jaa Nãa, nɩ a sorbo ba jaa Soro.
54006016	'Lɔ tɛɛ lɛ be be ba kpire ɛ, na wʋ be chãa 'lɔ pɔ nɩrɛ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ gbʋr ɛ, a 'lɔ nɩrɛ na ba nyɛrɛ ɛ, bɩɩ na tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ wʋ ɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ sɛɛn sɔ̃ɔ jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
54006017	A bala na ɩ a taraa dẽme a pʋ̃pãanyã, kpãa ba ɩka ba ta wile ba mɩ̃ɛ bɩɩ de a ba tɩɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a bʋ̃tarsɩ ala pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ ba dɩɛl Nãaŋmɩn nyã na kʋ sɩ a bʋ̃bʋrɔ bʋrɔsɩ a jaa a sɩ de chɩlɛ nɩ.
54006018	Kpãa ba a ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ vɩla na ba nʋ̃ɔ a vɩla tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ, na ba ɩ yɛ̃bɔ̃ɔnbɔ põnõ a ba bonsɩ.
