54006019	A lɛ ban bine na nãbonsɩ guro nɩ a nɩdaar, ka ba na nyɛ a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ nyɛvʋr.
54006020	A fʋ̃ʋ Timoti, gu a ala ban de 'yɔ̃ɔ a fʋ nũu pɔ, na fʋ bar a 'yɛrvor nɩ a nɛchɩrɛ ala na ba tara par ɛ, ban bʋɔlɔ a bɔ̃ɔfʋ,
54006021	bamɩne na kpãkpãana nɩ a yelsɩ anyãna, ba bar a sɔɔfʋ sɔr. Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋ be a fʋ sɛ̃.
55001001	Maa Pɔɔl na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nãa tu a Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ pɔ, nɩ a nɛɛ wʋn tɩr kʋ sɩ a nyɛvʋr nyã na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ,
55001002	sɛɛrɛ naa a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a fʋ̃ʋ Timoti na ɩ a n binʋ̃nãa. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ, nɩ nɩbaal, nɩ nyã'maar na yi a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jie wʋ be a fʋ sɛ̃.
55001003	N ma puor a Nãaŋmɩn nyã ɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ yãan nɩ a n tɩɛr wʋ jaa nɩtãa a lɛ a n sãakpãmɩne na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ, n maa ĩin a fʋ yele ɛ, naa ma tɩɛr fʋ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ fʋ tɩ̃sɔɔ nɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ.
55001004	N ma lɩɛb tɩɛr a fʋ nɩbikʋ̃ɔ fʋn ŋma, naa bʋɔrɔ ɩka n nyɛ fʋ ka a n pʋɔ pɛl.
55001005	N lɩɛb tɩɛr a fʋ yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔɔfʋ, a 'lɔ a fʋ makʋ̃ma Loisɩ nɩ a a fʋ ma Yunɩsɩ na dɔ̃ɔ tara, lɛ lɛ n mɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka fʋ mɩ tara wʋ naa.
55001006	A lɛ jũu, n lɩɛb tɩɛr fʋ ɩka fʋ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir fire a Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ 'lɔ na be a fʋ pɔ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ dɔɔl fʋ a n nuur ka fʋ nyɛ.
55001007	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wʋn kʋ sɩ ba ɩ dãbɩ̃ɛ Sɩɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ Sɩɛ 'lɔ na kʋ sɩ kpɛ̃ɔ ka sɩ tara nʋ̃fʋ, nɩ mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔfʋ.
55001008	Taa joro vɩ̃ nɩ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr mʋɔlfʋ ɛ, bɩɩ a maa ban pɔɔ a die pɔ a wʋ jũu ɛ, tɩchɛ pʋɔ ma a sɩ 'mataa dire a dɔɔyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ mʋɔlfʋ pɔ, na fʋ dɩɛl a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ.
55001009	'Lɔ lɛ faa sɩ na wʋ bʋɔl sɩ ɩka sɩ ɩ chɛchɛ, a ba ɩ a sɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ jũu lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a wʋ bɔfʋ nɩ a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu lɛ. Sɩ nyɛn a wɩ̃ɛfʋ nyã a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ tɩchɛ ka a wɛr wa maal.
55001010	Tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã, Nãaŋmɩn wiil sɩn a wɩ̃ɛfʋ nyã tu a sɩ Fafaara Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na wa a wɛr pɔ, na wʋ wa tʋ̃ɔ kũu tɩ na wʋ de a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ wiil sɩ a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
55001011	A 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyãna jũu lɛ wʋ ir ma ɩka n ɩ mʋmʋɔlɔ nɩ nɩtʋ̃nãa nɩ wiwile.
55001012	A anyãna jũu lɛ n dire a dɔɔyɛ, tɩchɛ vɩ̃ ba kpɛ ma ɛ, bojũu n bɔ̃ɔn a nɩrɛ 'lɔ ɩn sɔɔ naa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka wʋn gu ma naa tɩ tãn a bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a ala wʋn de 'yɔ̃ɔ a n nuur pɔ.
55001013	Nyɔɔ a 'yɛr sʋ̃ ala a lɛ nɛ fʋn wõ yi a n sɛ̃, a sɔɔfʋ nɩ a nʋ̃fʋ ala na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
55001014	Gu a yelmɩ̃ɛ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na de 'yɔ̃ɔ a fʋ nuur pɔ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sʋ̃ʋfʋ 'lɔ na be a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
55001015	Fʋ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a bala ba jaa na be a Asɩya tɔr man bar, Fɩgɛlusɩ nɩ Hɛmogɛnusɩ gba mɩ pʋɔ ba naa.
55001016	Nãaŋmɩn wʋ maal vɩla kʋ a Onesiforusɩ nɩ a wʋ yir dẽme, bojũu 'lɔ lɛ ma 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ma ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ, vɩ̃ ba kpɛ wʋ ɩn be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ jũu ɛ.
55001017	Wʋ gba na wa wa a Worom, wʋ yɔ bɔ man nɩbijɩɛ tɩ nyɛ ma.
55001018	A sɩ Soro wʋ sʋ̃ʋ wʋ a wʋ nyɛ maal vɩla a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ bɩbir daar. Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa a lɛ wʋn sʋ̃ʋ ma jɩ̃ be a Efesus.
55002001	Fʋ̃ʋ na ɩ a n bie, pãa kpɛ̃mɛ a wɩ̃ɛfʋ 'lɔ na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
55002002	A lɛ fʋn wõ a n sɛ̃ a nɩyɔɔ bala niem, de wiil a yelmɩ̃ɛ dẽme mɩ nɩ na tʋ̃ɔ wiil a ba taaba.
55002003	A fʋ̃ʋ mɩ, pʋɔ sɩ dire a dɔɔyɛ nɩtãa Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto soja mɩ̃ɛ.
55002004	A soja 'lɔ na be a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ, ma bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka a wʋ maalfʋ a pɛlɛ a 'lɔ na de wʋ a tʋ̃mɔ̃, maa lɛ tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ bere a bɩbir jaa yelbʋɔrsɩ pɔ ɛ.
55002005	Ala ɩ a bala na joro chɩrɛ taa bʋɔrɔ na ɩka ba dɔ̃ɔ a ba taaba, ba ma jon tu a lɛ ban wile.
55002006	A kʋɔraa 'lɔ na ba joro yãan ɛ, lɛ ma de a bʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ.
55002007	Tɩɛr kaa a lɛ ɩn 'yɛrɛ, bojũu a sɩ Soro na kʋ fʋ naa a jaa par bɔ̃ɔfʋ.
55002008	Tɩɛr a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ir a kũu pɔ, na yi a David bala pɔ. A anyãna lɛ ɩ a maa 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ mʋɔlfʋ,
55002009	a pɔ lɛ n dire a dɔɔyɛ, a ba wa lũ ma nɩ bɔ̃jɔrsɩ nɩdɛɛr kaar. Tɩchɛ baa tʋ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr lũ ɛ.
55002010	A lɛ jũu lɛ so, ka nyɔɔ n mɩ̃ɛ a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na ir jũu ka ba mɩ na nyɛ a faafʋ 'lɔ na be a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr.
55002011	A 'yɛr na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ nyã ɩka, ala ɩ sɩn nɩ 'lɔ lɛ 'mataa kpi, sɩn nɩ 'lɔ lɛ na 'mataa tara a nyɛvʋr.
55002012	Ala ɩ sɩ nyɔɔn sɩ mɩ̃ɛ, sɩn nɩ 'lɔ lɛ na 'mataa di a nãa. Ala ɩ sɩ chiir wʋ naa, wʋ mɩ na chiir sɩ naa.
55002013	Ala ɩ sɩn baa tara yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ 'lɔ chɛnɛ na tara yelmɩ̃ɛ, bojũu wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ chiir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
55002014	Mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir tɩɛrɛ ba a anyãna, na fʋ kpãana ba a Nãaŋmɩn niem ɩka, ba ta chɩrɛ taa nɩ a 'yɛrbie ɛ. A ba maala vɩla jaa ɛ, tɩchɛ a ma sɔ̃ɔn a bala na chɛlɛ tɩɛr.
55002015	Mɔ̃ na fʋ de fʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, an ɩ a 'lɔ mɩ̃ɛ lɛ pɛɛ fʋ, na fʋ ɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ 'lɔ na ba joro vĩ ɛ, na fʋ wile a yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr na tor.
55002016	Bar a nɛchɩrɛ ala na ba tara par ɛ, bojũu a lɛ na jãn nɩbɛ bar ka ba kʋ̃ lɛ ɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ɛ.
55002017	A ba wiilfʋ na yɔɔn gbõtor kaar. Hɩmɩnayas nɩ Filetusɩ mɩ pʋɔ ba naa.
55002018	Ba bar a yelmɩ̃ɛ tɩ 'yɛr ɩka kũu pɔ ir fʋ po naa, na ba sɔ̃ɔn bamɩne sɔɔfʋ.
55002019	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr par kparaa ara na, ka a sɛbie anyã sɛb a wʋ pɔ, "A sɩ Soro bɔ̃ɔn a bala jaa na ɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ." Na wʋ lɛ 'yɛr, "Vɛ̃ ka a bala jaa na bʋɔlɔ a sɩ Soro yuor, tɔɔ yɩ putuyele pɔ."
55002020	A yir kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ, bʋ̃dimaal bomo ma ben be, ka amɩne ɩ sɛlma, nɩ kpãna, tɩchɛ ka amɩne mɩ ɩ daar nɩ yɔɔraa, ka amɩne ɩ bʋ̃'yɔ̃ɔnsɩ, ka amɩne ɩ babãma bomo.
55002021	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ jaa na pɛɛn wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a bonsɩ anyã ɩn bʋɔl kaar, wʋn kaara na bʋ̃dimaal bomo na tara 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ na wʋ oo wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ a yir sʋɔ, ka wʋn tʋ̃ɔ de maal tʋ̃vɩla jaa bʋrɔ.
55002022	Tɔɔ yɩ a pɔlbil ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ pɔ, na fʋ turo yeltorsɩ, na fʋ tara sɔɔfʋ, nɩ nʋ̃fʋ, nɩ nyã'maar, 'matãan a bala na puoro a sɩ Soro nɩ a nyã chɛchɛ.
55002023	Tɔr a jɔl yele nɩ a nɛchɩrɛ na ba tara par ɛ, bojũu a maa yaara tɩ waan jɛɛr ɛ.
55002024	A ba sɛɛ ɩka a sɩ Soro tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ bʋɔrɔ jɛɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ maala vɩla kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa, na wʋ tʋ̃ɔ wile, na wʋ tara kãnyir.
55002025	A bala na chɩrɛ, wiil ba jomm, amɩne Nãaŋmɩn na wa sɔɔ naa ka ba lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr, na ba wa bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ.
55002026	Lɛ lɛ a ba tɩɛr na yuo a ba faa ba mɩ̃ɛ yin a Satan chɛbaa pɔ, a lɛ wʋn nyɔɔr ba a ba ɩrɛ a wʋ bɔfʋ.
55003001	Tɩchɛ bɔ̃ɔn a yele nyãna ɩka a bɩbir baaraa daar, dɔɔyɛ na ben be.
55003002	Nɩbɛ na nʋ̃n a ba mɩ̃ɛ, libinʋ̃nbɔ, mɩ̃ɛ 'mɔɔfʋ, ba kʋ̃ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩbɛ ɛ, na ba kʋ̃ wõnõ a ba dɔɔrbɔ toor ɛ, ka bon maa sɛɛ ba ɛ, na ba kʋ̃ ɩ chɛchɛ ɛ.
55003003	Ba maa tara nɩrɛ tɩɛr ɛ, ba maa vɛ̃ kʋ nɩrɛ ɛ, na ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa yoe, baa nyɔɔrɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, na ba 'yɛrɛ 'yɛrbikpɩ̃ɛn, na ba chire yelvɩla.
55003004	Ban ɩn gagarsɩ, na ba ɩ jukpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, na ba bʋɔrɔ yuor, ban nʋ̃n bʋ̃vɩɛlsɩ gar ban nʋ̃ Nãaŋmɩn,
55003005	ba maal ba mɩ̃ɛ Nãaŋmɩn puorbo kaar, tɩ chiir a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ. Ta gbɛɛrɛ ba ɛ.
55003006	A ba pɔ lɛ a bamɩne ma fara kpɩɛrɛ a yie pɔ na ba yʋɔrɔ bɛlɛ a pɔbɔ bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ a ba tɩɛr gaa jie ɛ, ka a ba yeldɛbɛ dɔl taa, ka a yeldɛbɛ jaa vɔlaa ma nyɔɔ ba.
55003007	Ba ma jãna na bɩbir jaa tɩ ba maa tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
55003008	Nɩtãa lɛ a Janɩsɩ nɩ Jãbɩrɛsɩ na ba sɔɔ a Mosesɩ ɛ, lɛ mɩ lɛ a nɩbɛ banyãna mɩ tɔr a yelmɩ̃ɛ, baa tara tɩɛr vɩla ɛ, a sɔɔfʋ yele jũu, ba ɩn faa.
55003009	A ba yele kʋ̃ chen tɛɛr ɛ, a lɛ an kaara a nɩbɛ ayi banyãna. Nɩrɛ jaa na nyɛn a lɛ ban jɔl jɩ̃.
55003010	Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ gba jaa nyɛn a n wiilfʋ bɔ̃ɔ, lɛ a n beraa na kaara, bon 'lɔ ɩn bʋɔrɔ a n nyɛvʋr pɔ, a n sɔɔfʋ, a n kãnyir, a n nʋ̃fʋ lɛ ɩn ara kpɛ̃ɔ,
55003011	a dɔɔyɛ ɩn di, nɩ a lɛ ban ge ma. Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa a lɛ na pɔɔ ma a Antiok, nɩ a Ikoniyum, nɩ a Lɩstɩra tẽn pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a sɩ Soro faa ma yin a jaa pɔ.
55003012	Sɩrɛ jaa, a bala jaa na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba turo a Nãaŋmɩn sɔr, na ba pɛlɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pʋɔ, na nyɛn gefʋ,
55003013	tɩchɛ a putudẽme nɩ a bala na maal ba mɩ̃ɛ nɩmɩn kaar, na kpɛ̃n sɔ̃ɔnaa pɔ, na ba wɛ, ba bɛlɛ naa ba taaba, ka ba kpɛ taa bɛlfʋ pɔ.
55003014	Fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ, mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nɩ a lɛ fʋn jãn na fʋ sɔɔ de, bojũu fʋ bɔ̃ɔn a nɩrɛ 'lɔ sɛ̃ fʋn jãn,
55003015	nɩ lɛ a fʋ bibile sɔ̃ɔ jaa fʋn bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn, na tʋ̃ɔ sʋ̃ʋ fʋ ka fʋ tara yɛ̃, nyɛ faafʋ, fʋn sɔɔ de a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jũu.
55003016	A Nãaŋmɩn gãma a jaa yi naa a wʋ sɛ̃, na a sɛɛ wiilfʋ, na a wile 'mabfʋ nɩ chɔɔrfʋ, naa na wiil nɩrɛ ka wʋ ɩ nɩtor.
55003017	Lɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩrɛ na bɔ̃ɔ na wʋ kpɛ̃mɛ kʋ tʋ̃vɩla jaa bʋrɔ.
55004001	N kpãana fʋ naa a Nãaŋmɩn niem nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na wa tɔɔr a kũn nɩ a vʋɛ 'yɛr, a wʋ waa daar, nɩ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ.
55004002	Mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr sɔ̃ɔ jaa, ka sɔr yuon bɩɩ ka sɔr ba yuo ɛ, kpãana ba, na fʋ wile, na fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn, na fʋ tara kãnyir wile nɩ.
55004003	Bojũu sɔ̃ɔ waara ka nɩbɛ kʋ̃ lɛ chɛlɛ a wiilfʋ ala na tor ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a ba tobo jɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba 'yɛryor wõfʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka ba bʋɔl wiwiilyɔɔ lɔ̃ɔtaar ka ba wile ba lɛ ban bʋɔrɔ.
55004004	Ban pãa lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ na ba chɛlɛ a wiilfʋ ala na ɩ jire.
55004005	Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, na fʋ tara kãnyir a fʋ dɔɔyɛ pɔ, na fʋ mʋɔlɔ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr, na fʋ tʋ̃ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ.
55004006	Bojũu a n nyɛvʋr nɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ ma ben baaraa ka n kʋ̃ yaar tɩ kpi ɛ.
55004007	Maa jɛb a jɛbvɩla, naa jo baar tun a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ, naa tara a sɔɔfʋ.
55004008	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a sɩ Soro na ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ tɔ tɔɔrɔ bin naa a nyɛvʋr nãa jupil gun ma, wʋn na kʋ ma a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, maa tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala jaa na nʋ̃ a wʋ waa.
55004009	Mɔ̃ wa a n sɛ̃ fɔfɔɔ jaa.
55004010	Bojũu Demas na nʋ̃ a dɩna wɛr jũu tɔr ma naa tɩ chen a Tɛsalonika, ka a Kɩrɩsɩn mɩ chen Galatiya ka Titusɩ mɩ chen Dalmatiya.
55004011	Luka tɛɛ lɛ be a n sɛ̃. Yɔbɔ Maakɩ ka yɩ 'mataa wa, bojũu wʋ tara na tɔ̃nɔ̃ na wʋn sʋ̃ʋ ma a tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ.
55004012	N tʋ̃n Tɩchɩkusɩ be a Efesus.
55004013	Fʋ̃ʋ wa waara, de a fuuvɛɛ 'lɔ ɩn bar be a Toroyas be a Kapusɩ sɛ̃ nɩ a gãma na fʋ 'mataa den a sɛɛr ala ban sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɛr gãn pɔ waan.
55004014	Aleksanda na ɩ a sãakuro maal man dɛɛr, a sɩ Soro na yab wʋn a lɛ wʋn maal ma.
55004015	Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ, bɔ̃ɔ a wʋ yele sʋ̃, bojũu wʋ chɩrɛ naa a lɛ sɩn 'yɛrɛ.
55004016	A dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ n 'yɛr faa a n mɩ̃ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa ba wa pʋɔ ma ɛ, tɩchɛ ba jaa tɔr man bar. Nãaŋmɩn wʋ ta de a lɛ yãan ba sãma ɛ.
55004017	Tɩchɛ a sɩ Soro ara na gu ma na wʋ kʋ ma kpɛ̃ɔ, ka a na tu a n 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a 'yɛrbir tʋ̃ɔ mʋɔl, ka a bala na ba puor ɛ, wõ naa. Lɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn faa ma a jukpɛ̃ɛ nɛɛ pɔ.
55004018	A sɩ Soro na faa man yin yelbier a jaa pɔ, na wʋ chiin ma a wʋ saaju nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ so a tɩɩr bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
55004019	Puor Pɩrɩsɩla nɩ Akuila, nɩ a Onesiforusɩ yir dẽme ba jaa.
55004020	Erastus chɛnɛ na be Korɩntɩ. Torofimusɩ an ɔɔrɔ ka n bar wʋ be Miletusɩ.
55004021	Mɔ̃ tɩ na fʋ wa tɩchɛ ka ɔɔr daar ta. Yubulus puoro fʋ naa nɩ Pudɛnsɩ nɩ Linus nɩ Kɩlaudiya nɩ a yɛɛr ba jaa.
55004022	A sɩ Soro wʋ be a fʋ sɛ̃, ka a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ be a yɩ jaa sɛ̃.
56001001	Maa Pɔɔl na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nãa, Nãaŋmɩn ir man tʋ̃ ɩka n tɩ sʋ̃ʋ a wʋ nɩchɛl irsɩ sɔɔfʋ ka ba bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ tɩ turo a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba turo.
56001002	Ala lɛ ɩ a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔn, a Nãaŋmɩn na ba ŋmaara jir ɛ, na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ sɩ a nyɛvʋr nyã yele sɛrɛ tɩ bon jaa wa piel.
56001003	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ na sɛɛ na wa ta, Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃ naa ka a wʋ 'yɛr gã chãa pɔ, ka n 'yɛrɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ a sɩ Fafaara na de kʋ ma ɩka n 'yɛr.
56001004	N sɛɛrɛ na a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a fʋ̃ʋ Titusɩ na sɔɔ a Yesu jũu, fʋ ɩ naa a n bie. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ sɩ Fafaara Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jie, a be a fʋ sɛ̃.
56001005	Lɛ na so ka n bar fʋ a Kɩrete paal nɩ nyã, ɩka fʋ baar maal a ala na chɛ ka a tor, tɩ na fʋ ir nɩbɛrɛ a tẽn ala nɩ tãa lɛ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ wiil fʋ.
56001006	A nɩdiere wʋ ta ɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ nɩbɛ na nyɛrɛ yeldɛbɛ a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, wʋ ɩ pɔɔ bʋ̃'yen sʋɔ, na wʋ ɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ a wʋ bibiir na sɔɔ Nãaŋmɩn, na ba ta ɩ bigãlsɩ nɩ bibawõnsɩ ɛ.
56001007	A nɩdiere an ɩ Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃mɔ̃ lɛ wʋ kaara jũu, wʋ ta ɩ tuor kʋ a nɩbɛ ɛ, wʋ ta ɩ nɩrɛ suur na ire fɔfɔɔ ɛ, na wʋ mɩ ta ɩ dãnburo ɛ, wʋ ta ɩ nɩrɛ na jɛɛrɛ, bɩɩ bʋɔrɔ libie na ba tu sɔr ɛ.
56001008	Wʋ ɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na diere sãanba, na wʋ nʋ̃ vɩla maalfʋ, na wʋ ɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nyɔɔrɔ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, na wʋ ma ɩrɛ a lɛ na tor, na wʋ ɩ nɩchɛchɛ, tɩ kpãana wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
56001009	Wʋ nyɔɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr nyã tara kpɛ̃ɔ nɩtãa lɛ an wiil. Lɛ lɛ wʋn tʋ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a bamɩne ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ wiilfʋ tɩ dɛn a bala na kpɛrɛ.
56001010	Bojũu a ba yɔɔ bala na ɩ a bawõnsɩ nɩ 'yɛr pɔrsɩ nɩ bɛ̃bɛlbɛ bala na yi a yɔŋmarba jie.
56001011	A sɛɛ naa ɩka fʋ ŋmaa ba sɔr, bojũu ba tu naa a ba bɔdɛbɛ bɛl yir gbulo nɩbɛ na ba wile yelsɩ ala na ba sɛɛ ɩka ba wile ɛ.
56001012	A ba yɛ̃ sʋɔ kɔ̃ɔ gba dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a ba 'yɛr, "Yɩn Kɩrete dẽme ɩn jir ŋmarba. Yɩ kaara fɩka dʋ̃dɛbɛ, koro dẽme na bʋɔrɔ bʋ̃diir tɛɛ."
56001013	A dãasɩɛ nyã ɩn sɩrɛ, a lɛ jũu, kpãa ba nɩbijɩɛ ka a ba sɔɔfʋ kpɛ̃mɛ a yelmɩ̃ɛ wiilfʋ pɔ,
56001014	ka ba ta chɛlɛ a Juu nɩbɛ fuolsɩ nɩ a bala na bar a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Ba tɔr a ba wiilfʋ.
56001015	Bala jaa na tara pʋtɩvɩla, yele jaa vɩla na kʋ ba, tɩchɛ bala na tara pʋtɩdɛɛr, na baa sɔɔ de ɛ, yele jaa ɩn dɛɛr a ba sɛ̃. Sɩrɛ jaa lɛ, a ba pʋtɩɛrsɩ dɛɛ naa.
56001016	Ba mɩ ɩka ba bɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn tɩchɛ a ba maalfʋ pɔ, ba tɔr wʋ naa. Ba ɩn nɩ'laarsɩ, bawõnsɩ na ba sɛɛn vɩla maalfʋ ɛ.
56002001	Fʋ̃ʋ Titusɩ, wile a nɩbɛ a lɛ na ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ wiilfʋ.
56002002	Wile a danyɔ̃n ka ba bal nɩbir, lɛ na vɛ̃ naa ka nɩbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba na ba nyɔɔrɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ, ka a ba sɔɔfʋ nɩ nʋ̃fʋ nɩ kãnyir tarfʋ chaar kʋ a nɩbɛ.
56002003	Lɛ mɩ lɛ, wile a pɔɔnyɔ̃n ka ba joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ na ba ta ɩ gagarsɩ ɛ, bɩɩ de ba ju 'yɔ̃ɔ dãa pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka ba wile a lɛ na vɩla.
56002004	Bala wa be a nɩtɔ̃, ban tʋ̃ɔn wile a pɔɔbil nɩ yɛ̃ ka ba nʋ̃ a ba sɩrbɛ nɩ a ba bibiir,
56002005	tɩ nyɔɔrɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ nɩ pʋpɛl, tɩ ɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ a yir na ba maala vɩla, tɩ turo a ba sɩrbɛ nɛɛ, ka nɩrɛ jaa ta nyɛ yeldɛɛr a ba Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr pɔ ɛ.
56002006	Lɛ mɩ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ, 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɔlbil ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn ka ba nyɔɔrɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ.
56002007	Yele jaa pɔ, vɛ̃ ka ba nyɛ a fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ maal vɩla jɩ̃nɛ. Vɛ̃ ka ba nyɛ a fʋ nɩbijɩɛ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ a fʋ wiilfʋ pɔ,
56002008	a fʋ 'yɛr na tor jũu, fʋ yuor kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɔ̃ɔ ɛ, ka a vĩ kpɛ a bala na kpɛrɛ fʋ, bojũu baa nyɛ 'yɛrdɛɛr jaa na 'yɛr a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
56002009	Wiil a gbãgbaar ka ba turo a ba nɩbɛrɛ nɛɛ yele jaa pɔ, na yɩ pɛl a ba pʋʋr na yɩ ta lɩɛrɛ ba nɛɛ ɛ.
56002010	Ba tara yelmɩ̃ɛ yele jaa pɔ, na ba ta juro a ba puor ɛ. Yɩn be ɩrɛ a lɛ, yele jaa yɩn maala, ban nyɛ naa a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ a sɩ yeldɛɛr Fafaara 'yɛr nʋ̃mɔ̃ a ba sɛ̃.
56002011	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn wiil sɩ naa a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ ka nɩrɛ jaa na tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ faafʋ.
56002012	A wile sɩ naa ka sɩ na tʋ̃ɔ lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ a ala Nãaŋmɩn na 'laar, bɩɩ vɛ̃ ka a wɛr nyã vɔlaa dib sɩ ɛ, tɩ kpɩɛrɛ nɩ mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔfʋ nɩ yeltorsɩ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ a dɩna wɛr nyã pɔ.
56002013	A lɛ sɩn chɛnɛ chɛlɛ ka a wɛr nyã pɔ, sɩ chɛnɛ na chɛlɛ a bɩbir kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a sɩ Fafaara na lɩɛb wa nɩ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ.
56002014	'Lɔ lɛ kpi a sɩ jũu na wʋ da sɩ faa sɩ yin a putuyele nyã pɔ, na wʋ pɛɛ a sɩ dɛbɛ bar ka sɩ ɩ wʋ mɩ̃ɛ nɩbɛ, ka vɩla maalfʋ ɩ sɩ vɔlaa.
56002015	Wile a anyãna, na fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔn ba ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn tɩ kpãana ba nɩbijɩɛ. Ta vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ jaa kaa fʋ pɔrɔ ɛ.
56003001	Tɩɛr a Yesu turbo ɩka ba turo a ba nɩbɛrɛ nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme nɛɛ tɩ turo a lɛ jaa ban 'yɛr, na ba chɔɔr gu vɩla jaa maalfʋ.
56003002	Ba ta ma ŋmara taa poe ɛ, tɩchɛ ba tara nyã'maar nɩ nɩrɛ jaa na ba tɩɛrɛ taa yele. Ba siir ba mɩ̃ɛ sɩrɛ jaa ka nɩbɛ nyɛ.
56003003	Sɩ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ jɔlɔ a ba kaar nɩ bawõnsɩ ka a Satan bɛl sɩ ka a wɛr nyã bonsɩ a jaa ma ɩrɛ sɩ vɔlaa, ka sɩ lɩɛb gbãgbaar, na sɩ pãa kpɩɛrɛ nɩ ger nɩ nyuur, ka ba 'laar sɩ, ka sɩ mɩ 'laar 'laar taa.
56003004	Tɩchɛ a sɔ̃ɔ na wa ta, a sɩ Fafaara Nãaŋmɩn maal vɩla nɩ a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ na wa wa,
56003005	wʋ faa sɩ naa, a ba ɩ a sɩ yelvɩɛl sɩn maal jũu ɛ, tɩchɛ a wʋ nɩbaal jũu lɛ. Wʋ faa sɩ naa na wʋ pɛɛ sɩ tu a dɔɔfʋ gbɛɛ ayi ka a wʋ Sɩɛ maal sɩ a sɩ ɩ nɩpaalaa,
56003006	a Sɩɛ nyã lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tu a Yesu na ɩ a sɩ Fafaara 'yɔ̃ɔ kʋ sɩ.
56003007	A lɛ lɛ, wʋn ben maal sɩ ka sɩ tor a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ jũu, sɩ ɩn a wʋ bʋ̃dirbe, na sɩ lɔb yãan bar guro nɩ a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
56003008	Yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr nɩ nyã, n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka fʋ do ara a yelsɩ anyãna pɔ wile nɩbijɩɛ, a lɛn vɛ̃ naa ka a bala na sɔɔ Nãaŋmɩn, de a ba sɔ̃ɔ nɩ a ba tɩɛr ɩrɛ nɩ yelvɩɛlsɩ tɛɛ. A lɛ vɩɛlɛ naa tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ nɩrɛ jaa.
56003009	Tɩchɛ ta chɛlɛ a jɔl chiirfʋ nɩ lɛ a sãakpãmɩne na tu taa mana bɩɩ jɛɛrɛ a nɛɛ 'lɔ ban bin a kõro jaa ɛ, bojũu a anyãna ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ.
56003010	Kpãa nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ooro gbɛbʋ̃'yen, 'lɔ wa tɔr, lɛ kpãa wʋ a gbɛɛ ayi sʋɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ wa tɔr, fʋ ir nũu tɩchɛ wʋ bar.
56003011	Fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a nɩrɛ nyã tɔ sʋɔ lo naa, wʋ mɩ̃ɛ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka wʋ ɩn dɛɛr.
56003012	N bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n tʋ̃ Atɩmasɩ bɩɩ Tɩchɩkusɩ a fʋ sɛ̃, ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na wa tɩ, mɔ̃ tɩ na fʋ tuor ma a be a Nikopolis, bojũu be lɛ n bʋɔrɔ ɩka n chen a ɔɔr sɔ̃ɔ.
56003013	Mɔ̃ na fʋ sʋ̃ʋ a 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ Jenasɩ nɩ Apolosɩ ka ba ta faa bon jaa a sɔr pɔ ɛ.
56003014	Vɛ̃ ka a sɩ nɩbɛ jãn vɩla maalfʋ ka ban tʋ̃ɔ maal a ala ban bʋɔrɔ na ba ta ɩ nɩhayasɩ ɛ.
56003015	Bala jaa na be ka a n sɛ̃, puoro fʋ naa. Puor a bala na nʋ̃ sɩ a sɔɔfʋ jũu. A wɩ̃ɛfʋ a be a yɩ jaa sɛ̃.
57001001	Maa Pɔɔl ban pɔɔ die pɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jũu nɩ Timoti na ɩ a sɩ yɛbɛ, lɛ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ a Filemon na ɩ a sɩ badatuo na wʋ ɩ a sɩ tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ,
57001002	na sɩ mɩ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ Afɩya na ɩ a sɩ yɛpɔɔ, nɩ Archipus na ɩ a sɩ soja ɩ̃sʋɔ, nɩ a pupuorbiir bala na ma 'lɔɔ a fʋ yir puor.
57001003	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na yi a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃, a be a fʋ sɛ̃.
57001004	N ma puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan sɔ̃ɔ jaa, naa ma pʋrɔ a fʋ yuor a n Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ pɔ,
57001005	bojũu n wõn a fʋ sɔɔfʋ fʋn tara a sɩ Soro Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ, nɩ a nʋ̃fʋ fʋn tara nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ba jaa.
57001006	N sʋɔrɔ na Nãaŋmɩn ɩka fʋ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir fʋ̃ʋ wa mana a sɔɔfʋ 'yɛr, na fʋ tara par bɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ a yelvɩɛl ala sɩn tara a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
57001007	N yɛbɛ, a fʋ nʋ̃fʋ vɛ̃n ka n chɩlɛ, na a 'yɔ̃ɔ ma ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ, bojũu fʋ 'maan a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ nyãn.
57001008	A lɛ jũu, ɩn naa tʋ̃ɔ chɛ nyãa a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ gba naa kpãa fʋ ɩka fʋ tʋ̃ a lɛ an sɛɛ ɩka fʋ tʋ̃,
57001009	tɩchɛ n sʋɔrɔ fʋ naa a nʋ̃fʋ jũu. Maa Pɔɔl pãa ɩn danyɔ̃ɔ, naa ɩ nɩrɛ ban pɔɔ die pɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jũu.
57001010	N sʋɔrɔ fʋ naa a Onɩsɩmɔsɩ na ɩ a maa bie, 'lɔ lɛ lɩɛb a n bie a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ban 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ.
57001011	A sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ, waa dɔ̃ɔ tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ fʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã wʋ tara na tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ a fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a maa.
57001012	N tʋ̃nɔ̃ wʋ naa, wʋ ɩn a maa mɩ̃ɛ nyãa ɩka wʋ lɩɛb wa a fʋ sɛ̃.
57001013	Ɩn taa nʋ̃n ɩka wʋ be a n sɛ̃ na wʋ ta de a fʋ jie sʋ̃nɔ̃ ma ban 'yɔ̃ɔ ma a bɔ̃jɔrsɩ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ mʋɔlfʋ jũu,
57001014	tɩchɛ n ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka n maal yele jaa ka maa ba sʋʋr fʋ kaa ɛ, ka a vɩla jaa na yi a fʋ nyãa pɔ naa taa ɩ fɩrfʋ ɛ.
57001015	Amɩne sɛ̃, ala lɛ tɔ̃ɔ so ka wʋ ŋmaa yi a fʋ sɛ̃ a bɩ̃lãa, tɩchɛ na wʋn lɛ wa be a fʋ sɛ̃ jaa kpo kpo.
57001016	Pʋ̃pãanyã waa lɛ chɛnɛ ɩ gbãgbaa ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ɩn gar gbãgbaa, na wʋ ɩ yɛbɛ kʋ fʋ. Wʋ ɩn nɩrɛ ɩn nʋ̃ ka fʋ mɩ gba nʋ̃, wʋn ɩ nɩrɛ nɩ yɛbɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ.
57001017	A lɛ jũu, ala ɩ fʋ nyɛ man ka n ɩ a fʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃tɔ sʋɔ, de wʋ nɩtãa a lɛ fʋn taa sɔɔ de ma.
57001018	Ala ɩ wʋ wa maal fʋn dɛɛr bɩɩ wʋ di fʋn sãn, de pʋɔ a maa sãn pɔ.
57001019	Maa Pɔɔl lɛ sɛɛrɛ a yele nyã nɩ a maa mɩ̃ɛ nũu. Ɩ̃n yab fʋ naa. N kʋ̃ 'yɛr 'yɛr jaa ɩka a fʋ̃ʋ mɩ̃ɛ gba mɩ di man sãn ɛ.
57001020	Ɔ̃ɔ, n yɛbɛ, vɛ̃ ka n nyɛ a tɔ̃nɔ̃ nyã yin a fʋ sɛ̃ a sɩ Soro 'yɔ̃ɔ, 'maa a n nyãa a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
57001021	N bar tɩɛr a fʋ nɛɛ tufʋ jũu, naa sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka fʋn maal gar a lɛ ɩn sʋɔr fʋ ɩka fʋ maal.
57001022	Yele bʋ̃'yen na chɛ, chɔɔr sãan gaa jie bar ma. A yɩ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ jũu, n tɩɛr ɩka wʋn sɔɔ naa ka a nɩbɛ banyãna yuo ma a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, ka n wa a yɩ sɛ̃.
57001023	Epafaras na ɩ a n tɔ sʋɔ ban 'mataa pɔɔ a die pɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jũu, puoro fʋ naa.
57001024	Ka Maakɩ mɩ nɩ Aristakus nɩ Demas nɩ Luka na ɩ a n taaba tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ, mɩ puoro fʋ naa.
57001025	A sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋ be a fʋ sɛ̃.
58001001	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ po, Nãaŋmɩn tun a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ sɛ̃ na wʋ 'yɛr 'yɛr dẽdẽme kʋ a sɩ sãamɩne sɔɩ yɔɔ jaa pɔ,
58001002	tɩchɛ a ber baaraa anyã 'lɔ, wʋ 'yɛr 'yɛr kʋ sɩ tun a wʋ Bie wʋn ir ka wʋn ɩ a bonsɩ a jaa bʋ̃dire. 'Lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ tu maal a wɛr wʋ jaa.
58001003	A Bie lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr chãa, na wʋ kaara a Nãaŋmɩn kaar jaa chɔ̃, ka a wʋ 'yɛr na tara kpɛ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ tɩɛn a bonsɩ a jaa taalɛ. A lɛ wʋn wa pɛɛ a yelbier baar, wʋ don tɩ jɩ̃nɛ a Tɩɩr Sʋɔ nũsʋ̃ɔ jie be a saaju.
58001004	Lɛ lɛ wʋ pãa gar a malakasɩ ba jaa, ka a yuor 'lɔ wʋn nyɛ, mɩ gar a ba bon.
58001005	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn ba dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ a malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ɩka, "Fʋ ɩn a n Bie, dɩna n lɩɛb a fʋ Sãa", bɩɩ 'yɛr go ɩka, "Ɩn ɩ naa a wʋ Sãa, ka wʋ mɩ ɩ a n Bie"?
58001006	A nɩ mɩ go, a lɛ wʋn waara nɩ a wʋ Bidadɔ̃ɔ ka a wɛr pɔ, wʋ 'yɛr naa, "Vɛ̃ ka a Nãaŋmɩn malakasɩ ba jaa gbur dumo puor wʋ."
58001007	A malakasɩ 'lɔ, nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn 'yɛr a ba 'yɛr, "Nãaŋmɩn maal a malakasɩ sɛsɛbɛ kaar. Ba ɩn a wʋ tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ kaara fɩka bũu 'lɩraa kaar."
58001008	Tɩchɛ, nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn gãn mɩ 'yɛr a Bie 'yɛr, "Nãaŋmɩn, a fʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ na ben be bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa, ka a torfʋ ɩ a fʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ dãgbal.
58001009	Fʋ nʋ̃n torfʋ tɩ na fʋ 'laar putuyele. A lɛ jũu, Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a fʋ Nãaŋmɩn, 'mɔɔ fʋ naa ka fʋ do gar a fʋ taaba ba jaa, a lɛ wʋn pʋr a pʋpɛl kãa 'yɔ̃ɔ fʋ."
58001010	A Nãaŋmɩn gãn lɛ 'yɛr naa, "A pielfʋ daar a fʋ̃ʋ Soro, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ kpar a tẽe par, ka a saaju wʋ jaa ɩ a fʋ nuur tʋ̃mɔ̃.
58001011	A jaa na wa sɔ̃ɔ naa, tɩchɛ ka fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ be be, a jaa na wa koraa naa chɩɛr fɔbaa kaar.
58001012	Fʋn pilãa naa fɩka fuu, naa lɩɛb fɔɔr kaar. Tɩchɛ ka a fʋ̃ʋ 'lɔ chɛnɛ a lɛ nɛ, ka a fʋ yuomo ba tara baarfʋ ɛ."
58001013	Malaka buor sʋɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ wa 'yɛr kʋ ɩka, "Jɩ̃nɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ jie, ka n wa de a fʋ dɔ̃dẽme ka ba ɩ a fʋ gbɛɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie"?
58001014	A ba ɩ a malakasɩ ba jaa ɩ naa a sɩtʋ̃nsɩ a Nãaŋmɩn na ma ir tʋ̃, ka ba wa sʋ̃nɔ̃ a bala na nyɛ a faafʋ ɛ?
58002001	Sɩ bɔ̃ɔ chɛlɛ sʋ̃, a lɛ jũu ka a bon 'lɔ sɩn wõ, ka sɩ taa sal lo ɛ.
58002002	Bojũu ala ɩ a malakasɩ 'yɛr ban dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ, ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na jɛb a 'yɛr bɩɩ tɔr a 'yɛr, ma nyɛn a toor tɔɔfʋ 'lɔ na tor,
58002003	ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a sɩn mɩ na ɩ chɩ̃ɛ, ala ɩ sɩ kaa naa a faa kpɛ̃ɛ nyã pɔrɔ? A sɩ Soro lɛ dɔ̃ɔ nie 'yɛr a faafʋ nyã 'yɛr, ka a bala na wõ naa pãa mɩ man jaa nɛ nɛ nɛ kʋ sɩ.
58002004	Nãaŋmɩn mɩ sɔɔ naa na wʋ de jɩ̃nsɩ, nɩ tʋ̃fɛrsɩ, nɩ nɛ'maa tʋ̃dẽdẽme, nɩ a lɛ wʋn kʋ sɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ, na wʋ kʋ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa a lɛ na ɩ a wʋ bɔfʋ.
58002005	A ba ɩ a malakasɩ lɛ na so a wɛr 'lɔ na waara ɛ, a 'lɔ 'yɛr sɩn ben 'yɛrɛ ɛ.
58002006	Tɩchɛ a jie ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'yɛr naa, "Bo lɛ nɩrɛ ɩ, ka fʋ tara a wʋ tɩɛr, bɩɩ nɩsaal bie mɩ ɩ ka fʋn tara a wʋ tɩɛr?
58002007	Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ maal wʋ, a wʋ ɩ jaa pʋʋr ka a malakasɩ gar wʋ, fʋ den tɩɩr nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋ wʋ.
58002008	Na fʋ de bonsɩ a jaa bin a wʋ gbɛɛ pĩlem." Nãaŋmɩn den bonsɩ a jaa kʋ wʋ, bon jaa ba be be ka waa tʋ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ. Tɩchɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã, saa nyɛ bonsɩ a jaa na siir ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ wʋ ɛ.
58002009	Tɩchɛ sɩ nyɛn a Yesu wʋn vɛ̃ ka wʋ ɩ jaa pʋʋr ka a malakasɩ gar wʋ, wʋ den tɩɩr nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ kʋ wʋ, bojũu wʋ din a kũu dɔɔyɛ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ vɛ̃ a wʋ lɛm kũu kaa kʋ nɩrɛ jaa.
58002010	Wʋn waara nɩ dabil yɔɔ a wʋ tɩɩr pɔ, a sɛɛn kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, a 'lɔ na so bonsɩ a jaa, nɩ a 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ bon jaa na tu be be, ka wʋ maal a ba nɩdɔ̃ɔn 'lɔ na faara ba ka wʋ ɩ chɛchɛ tu a wʋ dɔɔyɛ difʋ pɔ.
58002011	Ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na maala a nɩbɛ ka ba ɩrɛ chɛchɛ, nɩ a bala mɩ na ɩ a chɛchɛ ɩ sãa bʋ̃'yen bibiir. A lɛ jũu, vɩ̃ ba kʋrɔ a Yesu wʋn bʋɔlɔ ba yɛɛr ɛ,
58002012	na wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Ɩn pʋr a fʋ yuor kʋ a n yɛɛr, naa yiel yiel pɛɛn fʋ a bala na duo puoro fʋ niem."
58002013	A nɩ mɩ go, "Ɩn dɩɛl a n Nãaŋmɩn." Na wʋ lɛ 'yɛr go, "Maa nɩ nyã nɩ a bibiir bala a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ ma."
58002014	A bibiir na tara a ɩ̃gãn nɩ a jɩ̃ɩ jũu, ba mɩ dɔɔn a Yesu ka wʋ ɩ a ba ɩ̃sʋɔ, wʋ maal a lɛ, ka a wʋ kũu na tʋ̃ɔ sɔ̃ɔ a Satan nyã na tara a kũu kpɛ̃ɔ bar,
58002015	na wʋn faa a bala jaa bar ban dɔɔ, ka a kũu dãbɩ̃ɛ maal ba a ba lɩɛb gbãgbaar.
58002016	Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa a ba ɩ a malakasɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ waan a sʋ̃ʋfʋ nyã ɛ, tɩchɛ a Abraham yɔ̃n 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ.
58002017	Nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ jũu lɛ so, ka a Nãaŋmɩn maal wʋ a wʋ nyɛtãan a wʋ yɛɛr. Ka a lɛ vɛ̃ a wʋ ɩ nɩbaal kaara na wʋ ɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na tara yelmɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ, na wʋn tʋ̃ɔ de a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ lon a bɔɔr ka a nɩbɛ yeldɛɛr baar.
58002018	Bojũu a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ mɩ din tuo a bɛɛr kaa pɔ, wʋ mɩ na tʋ̃ɔn sʋ̃ʋ a bala jaa a bɛɛr kaa na nyɔɔ.
58003001	A lɛ jũu, yɛɛr na ba tara chɛfʋ ɛ, na yɩ pʋɔ a saaju bʋɔlfʋ pɔ, yɩ yuo a yɩ tɩɛr kʋ a Yesu, a nɩtʋ̃nãa nɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyã 'yɛr sɩn 'yɛrɛ.
58003002	Wʋ tara na yelmɩ̃ɛ kʋ a 'lɔ na ir wʋ, nɩtãa lɛ a Mosesɩ mɩ na dɔ̃ɔ tara yelmɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn yir wʋ jaa pɔ.
58003003	Yesu nyɛn 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ na sɛɛ na wʋ gar a Mosesɩ, nɩtãa lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na mɛ a yir na ma nyɛ a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ gar a yir mɩ̃ɛ.
58003004	Bojũu a yir jaa, nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ lɛ ma mɛ, tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ mɛ a bonsɩ a jaa.
58003005	Mosesɩ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃ na tara yelmɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn yir wʋ jaa pɔ, na wʋ dire a ala wʋn wa 'yɛr daar kɔ̃ɔ dãasɩɛ.
58003006	Tɩchɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, wʋ tara na yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn yir. Sɩn lɛ ɩ a wʋ yir, ala ɩ sɩ nyɔɔn nyãa nɩ a tɩɛrtɔfʋ 'lɔ sɩn bʋɔrɔ nɩ a yuor.
58003007	Lɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, "Dɩna ala ɩ fʋ wõn a Nãaŋmɩn kɔkɔr,
58003008	yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa kpɛ̃mɛ a yɩ nyãa nɩtãa lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ chɩɩr wʋ ɛ, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ bɛɛrɛ wʋ kaara be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ.
58003009	Be lɛ a yɩ sãakpãmɩne bɛɛr ma kaa na ba mɔ̃n ma lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩ tãn yuom lɩjaayi, na ba nyɛ a lɛ ɩn ɩ.
58003010	Ala lɛ so ka n nyɛn a nɩbɛ bala suur naa 'yɛr, 'A ba tɩɛrsɩ ma yɛ̃yɛlɛ naa. Baa bɔ̃ɔ a n sɔɩ ɛ.'
58003011	Lɛ lɛ, n nyɛn suur naa pɔ 'yɛr, 'Baa be jaa na wa kpɛ a n pɛ̃nfʋ pɔ go ɛ.' "
58003012	N yɛɛr, yɩ bɔ̃ɔ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa tara yeldɛɛr bɩɩ nyãa na ba sɔɔ de ɛ, na wʋ lɩɛb a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yin a Nãaŋmɩn na ba kpire sɛ̃ ɛ.
58003013	Tɩchɛ yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn bɩbir jaa, nɩtãa a bɩbir na chɛnɛ ka ba bʋɔlɔ a dɩna, ka yelbier taa bɛl ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ka wʋ kpɛ̃mɛ a wʋ nyãa ɛ.
58003014	Sɩ wa naa ka a sɩn nɩ a Kɩrɩsɩto na wa lɔ̃ɔ põ, ala ɩ sɩ ban gbɛr tɩ tãn a baaraa, a lɛ sɩn dɔ̃ɔ bar tɩɛr,
58003015	fɩka a lɛ an ben 'yɛr, "Dɩna, yɩn wa wõ a Nãaŋmɩn kɔkɔr, yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa kpɛ̃mɛ a yɩ nyãa ɛ, nɩtãa lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ chɩɩr wʋ ɛ."
58003016	Ba boo lɛ dɔ̃ɔ wõ tɩ chɩrɛ? A ba ɩ a bala Mosesɩ na dɔ̃ɔ tara yin a Ijipitɩ tẽe pɔ lɛ ɛ?
58003017	Ba boo mɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ nyɛn a suur a yuom lɩjaayi? A ba ɩ a bala na maal a dɛɛr ɛ, na ba lo kpi be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ lɛ ɛ?
58003018	Ba boo mɩ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pɔ 'yɛr ɩka ba kʋ̃ kpɛ a wʋ pɛ̃nfʋ jie ɛ, a ba ɩ a bala na dɔ̃ɔ tɔr a wʋ nɛɛ tufʋ bar lɛ ɛ?
58003019	Lɛ lɛ, sɩ nyɛn ban ba tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ɛ, bojũu baa tara sɔɔfʋ ɛ.
58004001	A lɛ jũu, an ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ a wʋ pɛ̃nfʋ pɔ kpɛfʋ na chɛnɛ be be, yɩ ɩ a sɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa wa kpɛ faa ɛ.
58004002	Bojũu a sɩn mɩ, ba mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ sɩ, nɩtãa lɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ ba. Tɩchɛ a 'yɛr ban dɔ̃ɔ mʋɔl kʋ ba, ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, bojũu a 'yɛr tɛɛ lɛ ba wõ, baa de sɔɔfʋ pʋɔ ɛ.
58004003	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a sɩn bala na sɔɔ de kpɛ̃n a pɛ̃nfʋ nyã pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, "N nyɛn suur naa pɔ 'yɛr, baa be jaa na wa kpɛ a n pɛ̃nfʋ pɔ go ɛ." Tɩchɛ wʋ tʋ̃n a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ baar yi a wɛr pielfʋ daar jaa.
58004004	Bojũu a jie ɩ̃sʋɔ wʋ 'yɛr naa a ber ayopõi daar 'yɛr, "A ber ayopõi daar, Nãaŋmɩn bar a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ a jaa tɩ pɛ̃n."
58004005	A 'yɛrbie anyãna nɩ a ju pɔ, wʋ lɛ 'yɛr naa, "Baa be jaa na wa kpɛ a n pɛ̃nfʋ pɔ ɛ."
58004006	Sɔr chɛnɛ na yuo ka bamɩne na kpɛ a pɛ̃nfʋ nyã pɔ, ka a bala ban de nie mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ nyã kʋ, ba tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ɛ, bojũu bawõnsɩ lɛ ba ɩ.
58004007	A lɛ jũu, Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ir bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ na wʋ bʋɔlɔ wʋ dɩna, a kor lɛ̃ɛɛ tɩchɛ a wʋ lɛ wa tu a Nãa David 'yɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a lɛ nɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, "Dɩna yɩn wa wõ a Nãaŋmɩn kɔkɔr, yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa kpɛ̃mɛ a yɩ nyãn ɛ."
58004008	Bojũu ala ɩ a Josua dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃ɔn a nɩbɛ kpɛ̃n a pɛ̃nfʋ nyã pɔ, Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ naa lɛ 'yɛr bɩbir ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr go ɛ.
58004009	A ber Ayopõi 'Lɔ Pɛ̃nfʋ chɛnɛ na be be kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ.
58004010	Bojũu nɩrɛ jaa na wa kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pɛ̃nfʋ nyã pɔ, wʋ mɩ ma pɛ̃n naa a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ na pɛ̃n a wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ.
58004011	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ɩ a sɩ mʋɔrɔ ɩka sɩ kpɛ a pɛ̃nfʋ nyã pɔ, ka nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa ɩ bawõno a ba kaar na wʋ bãr lo ɛ.
58004012	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɩn bʋ̃nɩbir, na wʋ ma pɩlpɩlɛ, na wʋ dire gar sɔbʋraa. Wʋ ma ŋmaan jaa kpɛ tɩ gbem a sɩɛ, na wʋ 'mar a kɔɔr, na wʋ wɛl a choofʋ jiir tɩ tãn a kɔɔr kãa pɔ. Wʋ ma tɔɔr tɩɛr nɩ befʋsɩ a jaa na be nɩrɛ nyãa pɔ 'yɛr.
58004013	Bon jaa ba be ka a bʋ̃maalsɩ pɔ naa sɔɔl a Nãaŋmɩn niem ɛ. Bon jaa ba pɔɔ ɛ, a jaa dɩɛl a wʋ niem. 'Lɔ lɛ sɩn wa man a yele a jaa kʋ.
58004014	A lɛ jũu, sɩn ben tara a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ na gar a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ ba jaa a wʋ do a be a saaju, Yesu na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, yɩ ɩ a sɩ ba gbɛr a sɩ sɔɔfʋ nyã sɩn sɔɔ pɔ.
58004015	Bojũu, saa tara a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kaa a sɩ balfʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩ tara na a 'lɔ mɩ a bɛɛr kaa bʋrɔ bʋrɔ na dɔ̃ɔ nyɔɔ a sɩn mɩ kaar, tɩchɛ waa ɩ yelbier ɛ.
58004016	Yɩ ɩ a sɩ daa yi a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ nãa dakɔɔ par nɩ nyãa, na sɩ tɩ de a wʋ nɩbaal na sɩ nyɛ wɩ̃ɛfʋ, ka a sʋ̃ʋ sɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ an wa wõnõ sɩ.
58005001	A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, ba ma kãan ir wʋ a nɩbɛ pɔ, na ba ir wʋ a wʋ ma ara kʋ ba nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sãlsɔɔ, na wʋ ma de a ba kʋfʋsɩ nɩ a ba bɔɔrlo bonsɩ loro nɩ a ba yeldɛbɛ bɔɔr.
58005002	Wʋ ma tʋ̃ɔn 'mʋ̃ɔn a bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩ chiine a jiyuo, bojũu a 'lɔ mɩ̃ɛ mɩ ba tara kpɛ̃ɔ ɛ.
58005003	A anyãna jũu lɛ so a wʋ ma de nie lo a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tulfʋ bɔɔr baar, tɩ pãa 'matãan a nɩbɛ ba jaa yeldɛbɛ bɔɔr.
58005004	Nɩrɛ jaa maa bʋ̃n kaa ir a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nyãna kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ma bʋɔl wʋ, nɩtãa lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔl a Aaron.
58005005	Lɛ mɩ lɛ, a Kɩrɩsɩto ba de a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nyã kʋ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ɛ, na wʋ wa lɩɛb a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɛ. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn mɩ lɛ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a n Bie, dɩna n lɩɛb a fʋ Sãa."
58005006	A lɛ 'yɛr a jie ɩ̃sʋɔ go, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a bɔɔrlo kpo kpo, nɩtãa a Melkijedek kaar."
58005007	A lɛ daar a Yesu na be ka a tẽe pɔ, wʋ den sʋɔrfʋ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kõn nɩbikʋ̃ɔ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na tʋ̃ɔ faa wʋ a kũu pɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn wõ a wʋ sʋɔrfʋ, bojũu wʋ den 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ siir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
58005008	Wʋ gba na ɩ a bie, wʋ jãn nɛɛ tufʋ yi a wʋ wõm pɔ.
58005009	Wʋn wa maal a lɛ an sɛɛ ɩka wʋ maal baar, wʋ lɩɛb a faafʋ sʋɔ kʋ a bala jaa na sɔɔ tu a wʋ nɛɛ.
58005010	Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ir wʋ a wʋ ɩ a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a Melkijedek kaar.
58005011	Sɩ tara na yɔɔ naa 'yɛr tun a yele anyãna pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a par wiilfʋ kpɛ̃mɛ, bojũu a yɩ bɔ̃ɔfʋ ba tal tɛɛr ɛ.
58005012	Yelmɩ̃ɛ, a sɛɛ naa a sɔ̃ɔ nyãna pɔ, ka yɩn taa ɩ wiwiilbe, tɩ yɩ chɛnɛ bʋɔrɔ nɩrɛ ɩka wʋ wiil yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbidɔ̃ɔ ala go. Bɩr lɛ yɩ chɛnɛ bʋɔrɔ, yaa ta saa difʋ ɛ.
58005013	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na chɛnɛ 'yɛnɛ bɩr, wʋ chɛnɛ na ɩ bipɩla. A wʋ yɛ̃ ba tal tɛɛr a wʋn tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a yeltorsɩ ban wile par ɛ.
58005014	Tɩchɛ nɩbɛrɛ bon lɛ saa, bala 'lɔ din nyɛ ka a mɩl ba, ka ba bɔ̃ɔ vɩla nɩ dɛɛr.
58006001	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ɩ a sɩ bar a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɛr pielfʋ yele, tɩ chiine niem lɩɛrɛ nɩbɛrɛ. Yɩ ta lɛ vɛ̃ ka sɩ pʋrɔ a tɩɛr lɩɛbfʋ yuor go ɛ, nɩ tʋ̃dɛɛr jaa bʋrɔ na chiine kũu pɔ ɛ, nɩ lɛ an sɛɛ ɩka fʋ tara a Nãaŋmɩn sɔɔfʋ,
58006002	nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ wiilfʋ, nɩ nuur dɔɔlfʋ yele, nɩ kũu pɔ irfʋ nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ yele.
58006003	Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn sɔɔ naa, sɩn ɩn a lɛ.
58006004	An ɩn tuo kʋ a bala na dɔ̃ɔ nyɛ a chãa, a bala na lɛm a saaju kʋfʋ kaa, na ba 'mataa põn a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ,
58006005	a bala na lɛm a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr vɩla kaa, nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ na waara a baaraa daar.
58006006	Ala ɩ ba faan lo, an ɩn tuo ka ba lɛ waan ba a ba wa nyɛ tɩɛr lɩɛbfʋ, bojũu a ba bɔrfʋ lɛ kpara naa a Nãaŋmɩn Bie a daa ju go, na ba lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ ka a nɩyɔɔ lɛ wuolo wʋ.
58006007	A lɛ a tẽe na ma nyũ a sabie kʋ̃ɔ na ma loro na wʋ bul a bonsɩ ala na tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ a bala na kɔ, ma nyɛn a Nãaŋmɩn sʋ̃ʋfʋ.
58006008	Tɩchɛ a tẽe 'lɔ na ma bul a gʋʋr nɩ a mɔ-ur, waa tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ ɛ, tɩ na wʋ be pɔ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ. A baarfʋ daar bũu lɛ na di wʋ.
58006009	Sɩ gban 'yɛrɛ a anyãna, barmɩne, sɩ bar tɩɛr a yɩ jie, na sɩ bɔ̃ɔn yɩn tara bʋ̃sʋ̃n, bʋ̃sʋ̃n ala na lɔ̃ɔn a faafʋ.
58006010	Nãaŋmɩn ba ɩ nɩbur bur ɛ. Wʋ kʋ̃ ĩin a yɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ a yɩ nʋ̃fʋ yɩn wiil kʋ wʋ ɛ, na yɩ sʋ̃ʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ tɩ chɛnɛ sʋ̃nɔ̃ ba.
58006011	Sɩ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir maala a lɛ nɛ tɩ tãn a baaraa, na yɩ kʋ̃ baala a yɩ tɩɛrtɔ jie ɛ.
58006012	Saa bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ ɩ koro dẽme ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ tɔɔrɔ a bala na tu a sɔɔfʋ pɔ tara kãnyir nyɛn a bonsɩ ala a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ.
58006013	Lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩrɛ a nɛɛ kʋrɔ a Abraham, nɩrɛ jaa na ba be be gar wʋ a wʋn pɔn jũu, wʋ pɔn naa a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ,
58006014	na wʋ 'yɛrɛ, "Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ, ɩn sʋ̃ʋ fʋ naa, naa vɛ̃ ka a fʋ bal par paal."
58006015	Lɛ lɛ a Abraham tara a kãnyir na wʋ chɛl lɛ̃ɛɛ wa de a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ wʋ.
58006016	Nɩrɛ ma den a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na gar wʋ yuor pɔn, ka a lɛ wʋn ma tɩr a nɛɛ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, ka a wɩlɛwɩlɛ maa lɛ be be go ɛ.
58006017	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ maal a wʋ befʋ 'lɔ na ba lɩɛrɛ ɛ, ka a chaar kʋ a bala na wa de a ala wʋn tɩr a nɛɛ. Wʋ tɩr nɛɛ ɩka wʋn maal a lɛ.
58006018	Nãaŋmɩn maal a nɩtɔ̃ ɩka, a bonsɩ ayi anyã na ba tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ lɩɛrɛ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn mɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ŋmaa jire ɛ, ka a sɩn bala na jo tɩ nyɔɔ a tɩɛrtɔfʋ nyã wʋn kʋ sɩ a pɔrɔ taalɛ, ka a na 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn.
58006019	A tɩɛrtɔfʋ nyã lɛ sɩ tara, naa ɩ a nɛbikur na ma lũ a sɩ sɩɛ a wʋ chɩm ba dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ. Wʋ põn kpɛ be a diniem a fɔbaa 'lɔ ban lũ var puor.
58006020	Be lɛ a Yesu de nie chen a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, wʋ kpɛ naa a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ. Wʋ ɩ naa a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ kpo kpo nɩtãa a Melkijedek kaar.
58007001	A Melkijedek nyã lɛ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a Salem nãa nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn na do gar a saaju bɔɔrloro. 'Lɔ lɛ tuor a Abraham na wʋ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ, a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ jɛb a nãmɩne bala tʋ̃ɔ tɩ lɩɛb waara.
58007002	Ka a Abraham ir a bonsɩ ala wʋn waara nɩ a jaa pɔ pie, bʋ̃'yen kʋ wʋ. A wʋ yodɔ̃ɔ par nɩ nyã, torfʋ nãa, a nɩ mɩ, Salem nãa, a par lɛ, nyã'maar nãa.
58007003	Waa tara sãa ɛ, bɩɩ ma ɛ, nɩrɛ jaa ba bɔ̃ɔ a wʋ dɔɔfʋ daar ɛ, bɩɩ bɔ̃ɔ a wʋ bal par ɛ, bɩɩ a wʋ kũu daar ɛ. Wʋ kaara naa a Nãaŋmɩn Bie kaar, na wʋ ɩ a bɔɔrlo kpo kpo.
58007004	Yɩ tɩɛr kaa a lɛ wʋn bɛrma jɩ̃. A sɩ sãakpã Abraham gba mɩ dɔ̃ɔ kʋ wʋ a bonsɩ ala wʋn fa pɔ pie jaa pɔ bʋ̃'yen.
58007005	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a Mosesɩ nɛɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ bin 'yɛr naa ɩka, a Levi bal par pɔ lɛ a bɔɔrloro na ma yi, 'lɔ lɛ na ma de a pie jaa pɔ bʋ̃'yen yin a Isɩral nɩbɛ ba jaa sɛ̃, a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yɛɛr sɛ̃, a ba yɛɛr gba mɩ na ɩ a Abraham bal nɩbɛ sɛ̃.
58007006	Tɩchɛ a daba nyã baa gba bɩɛr a wʋ tɩ yi a Levi bal par pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ den a pie pɔ bʋ̃'yen yi a Abraham sɛ̃, na wʋ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ a 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛr kʋ.
58007007	Baal ba be be ɛ, ɩka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na bɛrmɛ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ a 'lɔ na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ.
58007008	A yele ɩ̃sʋɔ nɩ nyã ɩka, a bala na kpire lɛ ma de a pie pɔ jaa bʋ̃'yen, tɩchɛ a sɔr ɩ̃sʋɔ pɔ, a Melkijedek 'lɔ na ba kpire ɛ, de naa.
58007009	Ɩ̃sʋɔ gba mɩ na 'yɛr ɩka, a Levi nɩrɛ na ma de a pie jaa pɔ bʋ̃'yen, ba yab a pie jaa pɔ bʋ̃'yen tu a Abraham sɛ̃,
58007010	bojũu a lɛ a Melkijedek na dɔ̃ɔ tuor a Abraham, a Levi chɛnɛ na be a wʋ sãakpã pʋɔm.
58007011	Ala ɩ a Levi bal nɩrɛ, a bɔɔrlo tʋ̃mɔ̃ ma ta vɛ̃n ka wʋ tor jaa dẽ dẽ, a nɛbinãa 'lɔ ban kʋ a nɩbɛ, bo lɛ so ka ba lɛ bʋɔrɔ a bɔɔrloro ɩ̃sʋɔ ɩka wʋ wa, na wʋ kaara a Melkijedek kaar na waa ɩ a Aaron kaar ɛ?
58007012	Bojũu bala wa lɩɛr a bɔɔrloro, ba mɩ ma lɩɛr a nɛbinãa.
58007013	A 'lɔ ban 'yɛrɛ na so a yele anyãna, wʋ ɩn bal yuo, ka nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba yi a bala nyãna pɔ na wʋ tɩ tʋ̃ tʋ̃mɔ̃ be a bɔɔr lofʋ jie ɛ.
58007014	Bojũu nɩrɛ jaa bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a sɩ Soro ɩn a Juda bal nɩrɛ, ka a bala nyã pɔ, Mosesɩ mɩ ba pʋr a yuor ɩka nɩrɛ na yin a bala nyã pɔ tɩ ɩ a bɔɔrloro ɛ.
58007015	Ka a lɛ sɩn 'yɛr gba gãn chãa pɔ, ɩka ala ɩ a bɔɔrloro ɩ̃sʋɔ na kaara a Melkijedek kaar wa wa naa,
58007016	a 'lɔ na wa ɩ a bɔɔrloro 'lɔ na ba tu a lɛ a nɛbinãa na 'yɛr tun a wʋ sãakpã loor ɛ, tɩchɛ a tun a lɛ a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ na yi a nyɛvʋr na ba tara sɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ.
58007017	Bojũu a sɛb ɩka, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a bɔɔrlo kpo kpo na ba tara tɛɛfʋ ɛ, nɩtãa a Melkijedek."
58007018	Ba tɔɔn a kõro binfʋ lan bar, bojũu wʋ bal naa na waa ɩ bʋ̃joraa go ɛ.
58007019	Bojũu a nɛbinãa nyã maa tʋ̃ɔ maal bon ka wʋ tor jaa dẽ dẽ ɛ, ka a tɩɛrtɔ yuo na ɩ gar wʋ wa, na wʋ vɛ̃ ka sɩ tɔɔ gbʋr Nãaŋmɩn.
58007020	A Nãaŋmɩn nɛtɩraa dɔ̃ɔ be be, bamɩne lɩɛb a bɔɔrlorbo ka a nɛtɩraa ba pʋɔ ɛ,
58007021	tɩchɛ 'lɔ lɩɛb a bɔɔrloro ka a nɛtɩraa pʋɔ, a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "A sɩ Soro pɔn 'yɛr, na wʋ kʋ̃ wa puur a kʋ̃ɔ bar jaa ɛ. Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a bɔɔrlo kpo kpo."
58007022	A pɔ binfʋ nyãna jũu, Yesu lɛ wʋ de bin a nɛɛ ka wʋ ɩ a nɛtɩraa na gar.
58007023	A kõro a bɔɔrlorbo bala ma dɔ̃ɔ ɩ yɔɔ, bojũu kũu maa sɔɔ ka ba be be a tʋ̃mɔ̃ pɔ kor ɛ.
58007024	Tɩchɛ a Yesu 'lɔ na ben be jaa kpo kpo, a wʋ bɔɔrlo tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba tara lɩɛrfʋ ɛ.
58007025	A lɛ jũu, wʋ ma tʋ̃ɔn faa a bala na tu a wʋ jie waara a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃. Bojũu wʋ ma ben be sɔ̃ɔ jaa 'maala a Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ ba.
58007026	A bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyãna lɛ bɔ̃ɔ a lɛ sɩn bʋɔrɔ, wʋ ɩn chɛchɛ, waa tara chɛfʋ ɛ, waa bʋɔrɔ yeldɛɛr ɛ, na wʋ oo wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yin yelbe-ɩrbɛ pɔ, na wʋ do gar a saaju.
58007027	Waa kaara fɩka a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ banyã ɛ, naa ba lɛ sɛɛ ɩka wʋ loro a bɔɔr a bɩbie a jaa ɛ, na wʋn ma de nie lo a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tulo bɔɔr, tɩ pãa mɩ lo a nɩbɛ mɩ bon ɛ. Wʋ mɩ̃ɛ lɛ sɔɔ na wʋ lɩɛb a bɔɔrlo dʋ̃ɔ lo a ba yeldɛbɛ bɔɔr a dẽdẽe daa ka a baar.
58007028	Bojũu a nɛbinãa lɛ ma ir a bɔɔrlo nɩbɛrɛ, ka ba ɩ nɩbɛ na bal, tɩchɛ a pɔfʋ nyã na tu a nɛbinãa puor wa, a Bie lɛ Nãaŋmɩn ir, 'lɔ lɛ maal a lɛ jaa a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ maal.
58008001	A 'yɛrɛ sɩn 'yɛrɛ nɩ nyã, sɩn tara na a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyã na jɩ̃nɛ be a saaju kpɛ̃ɔ wʋ jaa sʋɔ nũsʋ̃ɔ jie.
58008002	Be lɛ wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a dinie sʋɔ na ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir a sɩ Soro mɩ̃ɛ na maal, a ba ɩ a gãn yir 'lɔ a nɩrɛ na maal a wʋ nũu ɛ.
58008003	Bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ jaa ba ma ir wʋ naa ka wʋ ma diere a kʋfʋsɩ nɩ a bɔɔrlo bonsɩ loro nɩ a bɔɔr, ala lɛ so ka a nyã mɩ na de bon kɔ̃ɔ lon a bɔɔr.
58008004	Ala ɩ wʋ ta ben ka a tẽe pɔ, wʋ kʋ̃ naa ta ɩ bɔɔrloro ɛ, bojũu nɩbɛ den nie be ka, na ba ma diere a kʋfʋsɩ turo nɩ a lɛ a nɛbinãa na man.
58008005	Ban tʋ̃nɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir chɛchɛ nyã pɔ na ɩ a 'lɔ na be a saaju gãagiel ban tɔɔr maal. A anyãna jũu lɛ so ka a Nãaŋmɩn kpãkpãana a Mosesɩ a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ maal a gãn yir, na wʋ 'yɛr, "Kaara sʋ̃, na fʋ maal wʋ a lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju ɩn wiil fʋ be a tɔ̃ɔ ju."
58008006	Tɩchɛ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ 'lɔ a Yesu na nyɛ, gar a ba bon jaa bamm na ɩ a nɛtɩraa 'ma'maala na gar a bʋ̃koraa, bojũu a nɛbin paalaa na ɩ gar pɔ lɛ wʋ maal.
58008007	Bojũu ala ɩ a nɛtɩr koraa 'lɔ ba dɔ̃ɔ tara chɛfʋ ɛ, jie kʋ̃ naa be be a ba lɛ bʋɔrɔ bʋ̃yuo ɛ.
58008008	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn nyɛn a lɛ a nɩbɛ na 'mab, na wʋ 'yɛr, nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr, "Bɩbir kɔ̃ɔ na wa vɩɛ naa, ka n tɩr nɛtɩr paalaa bin kʋ a Isɩral yir dẽme nɩ a Juda yir dẽme.
58008009	A kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛtãan a nɛɛ 'lɔ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ tɩr kʋ a ba sãakpãmɩne a daar 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩn nyɔɔ ba a nũu tɔɔ yin a Ijipitɩ tẽe pɔ ɛ. Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr, bojũu baa sɔɔ ara a lɛ ɩn tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ ba ɛ, ka n mɩ lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ ba.
58008010	A anyãna lɛ ɩ a nɛtɩraa ɩn na tɩr kʋ a Isɩral yir dẽme, a bɩbir 'lɔ wa vɩɛ baar. Lɛ lɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr. Ɩn de naa a n nɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba tɩɛrsɩ pɔ, na n sɛb dɔɔl a ba nyãn ju. Ka n ɩ a ba Nãaŋmɩn, ka ba mɩ ɩ a n nɩbɛ.
58008011	Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ lɛ wiil a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ ɛ, bɩɩ ka nɩrɛ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ yɛbɛ ɩka, 'Bɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro ɛ.' Bojũu ba jaa na bɔ̃ɔ ma naa, yi a bil pɔ tɩ tãn a bɛrɛ pɔ.
58008012	Ɩn vɛ̃n a ba putuyele bar. N kʋ̃ lɛ tɩɛr a ba yeldɛbɛ jaa go ɛ."
58008013	Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔlɔ a nɛtɩraa anyãna bʋ̃paalaa, wʋ maal a 'lɔ na de nie ka wʋ ɩ bʋ̃jʋɔlaa, ka bon mɩ na jʋɔl, wʋ maa yaara tɩ kpi ɛ.
58009001	Faa nyɛ, a nɛtɩr dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ tara na a puorfʋ chirsɩ nɩ a jichɛchɛ 'lɔ ban dɔ̃ɔ maal ka a tẽe pɔ.
58009002	A gãn yir nyã ban dɔ̃ɔ maal baar, a di yɛ̃yɛ̃ pɔ lɛ ba bin a fɩ̃tɩnsɩ dɔɔlfʋ jie nɩ a tɛɛbʋl 'lɔ ju ban ma dɔɔl a paanʋ̃chɛchɛ ala. A jie nyã lɛ ba bʋɔlɔ, Jichɛchɛ.
58009003	A dinie sʋɔ ban lũ a fɔbaa var, ba bʋɔlɔ naa a be, Chɛchɛ wʋ jaa Chɛchɛ Jie.
58009004	Be lɛ a bɔɔr lofʋ jie be na ɩ sɛlma a ba ma chʋnɔ̃ a tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla ala nɩ a nɛtɩraa daka ban maal tɩ waar sɛlma pɔɔ. A daka nyãna pɔ lɛ a sɛlma dulo ban 'yɔ̃ɔ a maana nɩ a Aaron dãgbal 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ 'mʋr a puul nɩ a kʋsɩr pɛ̃rsɩ ala ban dɔ̃ɔ sɛb a nɛbinãa 'yɔ̃ɔ.
58009005	A daka nyã ju lɛ ba maal a malakasɩ bala na wile a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr ka ba ara kʋ a malakasɩ bala ban bʋɔlɔ a cherubim, ka ba ger pɔɔ a faafʋ bɔɔr lofʋ jie. Tɩchɛ sɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ man a yelsɩ anyãna tu tu taa a pʋ̃pãanyã ɛ.
58009006	Lɛ a yelsɩ anyãna ban wa chɔɔr a nɩtɔ̃ baar, a bɔɔrlorbo pãa ma kpɩɛrɛ na a di yɛ̃yɛ̃ sʋɔ pɔ, bɩbir jaa tʋ̃nɔ̃ a ba tʋ̃mɔ̃.
58009007	Tɩchɛ a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ tɛɛ lɛ ma kpɛ a dinie sɔɔ gbɛbʋ̃'yen yuon jaa, wʋ maa faa dʋ̃ɔ jɩ̃ɩ ɛ. Ala lɛ wʋ ma kpɛ̃n a be tɩ lon a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ bɔɔr, nɩ a nɩbɛ mɩ yeldɛbɛ ban ba bɔ̃ɔn ɛ, tɩ faa tul maal bɔɔr.
58009008	Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wiil a anyãna ɩka, a sɔr na kpɩɛrɛ a Jichɛchɛ 'Lɔ Wʋ Jaa Chɛchɛ Jie chɛnɛ na ba yuo ɛ, a gãn yir koro na chɛnɛ ara jũu.
58009009	A anyãna dɔ̃ɔ wile a dɩna sɔ̃ɔ, naa wile ɩka a kʋfʋsɩ nɩ a bɔɔrlo bonsɩ ala ban ma lon a bɔɔr, maa tʋ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka a 'lɔ na wa a puorfʋ jie tɩɛr chaar ɛ.
58009010	A ɩ naa bʋ̃diir tɛɛ yele, nɩ nyũfʋ yele, nɩ bʋ̃pɛɛrsɩ yelsɩ, ala lɛ ba mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir maala tɩ tãn a yelpaalaa na lɩɛr.
58009011	Lɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na wa a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyã kaar, nɩ a yelsʋ̃n ala na de nie be ka, wʋ kpɛ̃n tu a jikpɛ̃ɛ nɩ a puorfʋ yir 'lɔ na ɩ chɛchɛ an ba ɩ nɩrɛ nũu lɛ maal ɛ, ka sɩ 'yɛr ɩka waa pʋɔ a bʋ̃mɩɛrsɩ pɔ ɛ.
58009012	Waa de bʋɔ bɩɩ narbil jɩ̃ɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ kpɛ naa a Jichɛchɛ Wʋ Jaa Chɛchɛ nyã pɔ, gbɛbʋ̃'yen kʋ nɩrɛ jaa nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ jɩ̃ɩ, a sɩ tɔ̃ɔ nyɛ a faafʋ a kpo kpo.
58009013	A bʋʋr jɩ̃ɩ nɩ a nadai jɩ̃ɩ nɩ a nasarbil tãpɩɛl ban ma ɔ̃ɔ mɩr a bala na sɔ̃ɔ, ka a ba ɩ̃gãma yi ɩ bʋ̃sʋ̃n.
58009014	Ŋmɩnɛ pãa lɛ, a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto jɩ̃ɩ a 'lɔ na tu a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na ɩ nyɛvʋr, a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ na ba tara chɛfʋ ɛ, lon bɔɔr kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn na wʋ pɛɛ a sɩ tɩɛr nɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ jaa na chiine nɩ sɩ kũu pɔ, ka sɩn tʋ̃ɔ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn vʋr.
58009015	Bojũu a anyãna lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ɩ a nɛtɩr paalaa 'ma'maala, ka a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl, na nyɛ a bʋ̃sʋ̃n ala na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. Pʋ̃pãanyã wʋ kpi naa na wʋ faa ba yin a yeldɛbɛ ala ban dɔ̃ɔ maal a nɛtɩr koraa 'lɔ pɔ.
58009016	Nɩrɛ wa tɩr nɛɛ ɩka 'lɔ wa kpi baar, a kũu lɛ wʋ ma wa kpi, ka a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr pãa yi chãa pɔ,
58009017	bojũu ala ɩ fʋ tɩr nɛɛ ɩka fʋ̃ʋ wa kpi baar. Fʋ̃ʋ wa chɛnɛ a ba ɩ yele ɛ, tɩchɛ fʋn wa kpi baar lɛ a pãa ɩ yele.
58009018	A anyãna jũu lɛ so gba, ka a nɛtɩr dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ maa ɩ bon jaa ka a jɩ̃ɩ ba pʋɔ ɛ.
58009019	Lɛ a Mosesɩ na wa man a nɛbinãa 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbɛ ba jaa baar, wʋ den a nelpɔlɔ jɩ̃ɩ na wʋ de kʋ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ, na wʋ de pɛr kɔɔl jɩɛ na wʋ vʋ̃ɔ urbanyũu na wʋ tun mɩr a gãn pilãa 'lɔ nɩ a nɩbɛ ba jaa.
58009020	Tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, "A anyãna lɛ ɩ a nɛtɩraa jɩ̃ɩ, a Nãaŋmɩn na kpãkpãana yɩ ɩka yɩ turo."
58009021	Lɛ nɩ ju mɩ lɛ wʋ de a jɩ̃ɩ mɩr a gãn puorfʋ yir nɩ a bonsɩ a jaa ban ma de maala nɩ a be.
58009022	Yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa a nɛbinãa 'yɛr ɩka, ba ma de a jɩ̃ɩ mɩɩl a bonsɩ a jaa. Ka jɩ̃ɩ ba wa kpaar ɛ, yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ ba be be ɛ.
58009023	A tara na sɔr ka ba chɔɔr a saaju bʋ̃tɔɔr maalaa nɩ a bɔɔrlo bonsɩ anyãna, tɩchɛ a saaju bonsɩ mɩ̃ɛ 'lɔ, a ba bɔɔrlo bon gar naa anyãna.
58009024	Bojũu Kɩrɩsɩto ba kpɛ a nɩrɛ nũu bʋ̃maalaa jichɛchɛ nyã pɔ, na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a saaju bon sʋ̃ 'lɔ ban dɔ̃ɔ tɔɔr maal ɛ. A saaju mɩ̃ɛ lɛ wʋ tɩ kpɛ, na wʋ tɩ ara a Nãaŋmɩn niem a pʋ̃pãanyã a sɩ jũu.
58009025	A ba ɩ wʋ kpɛ̃n be a saaju na wʋn lɛ tɩ loro a bɔɔr bɩbir jaa ɛ, nɩtãa lɛ a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlo nãa na ma kpɛ a Jichɛchɛ 'Lɔ Wʋ Jaa Chɛchɛ pɔ, a yuon nɩ a jɩ̃ɩ na ba ɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ jɩ̃ɩ ɛ.
58009026	Ala ɩ lɛ lɛ a ta ɩ, Kɩrɩsɩto naa pãan din dɔɔyɛ sɔ̃ɔ jaa yi a wɛr pielfʋ daar jaa. Tɩchɛ a pʋ̃pãanyã, wʋ wa daan yi a bɩbir baaraa daar na wʋ maal yele a jaa baar, ɩka wʋ wa de a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ lɩɛb a bɔɔrlo bon diin a yelbier bar.
58009027	Nɩtãa lɛ ban dɔɔ nɩrɛ ka wʋn kpi daar kɔ̃ɔ, na wʋ tɩ tuor 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ,
58009028	lɛ lɛ, a Kɩrɩsɩto lon a bɔɔr kpo kpo kʋ nɩyɔɔ. Wʋn lɩɛb wa a gbɛɛ ayi sɔ̃ɔ, a ba ɩ fɩka a wʋ wa de a yelbier bar ɛ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ waan faafʋ wa kʋ a bala jaa na chɛlɛ wʋ.
58010001	A nɛbinãa dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a bʋ̃sʋ̃ 'lɔ na waara gãagiel, a ba ɩ a bon mɩ̃ɛ lɛ ɛ. A nɩtɔ̃ jũu, a kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ɩ a bɔɔrlo bʋ̃bʋ̃'yen ban ma lo yuon jaa ka a tʋ̃ɔ chɔɔr a bala na ma wa tɔɔ gbʋr a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
58010002	Ala ɩ a ta tʋ̃ɔn chɔɔr ba, ba kʋ̃ naa bar a bɔɔrlo bomo ir fʋ ɛ? Bojũu a bala na ma ta wa a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ jie, a ba yelbier naa baar naa, ka ba kʋ̃ ma lɛ tɩɛr tɔ a ba yeldɛbɛ go ɛ.
58010003	Tɩchɛ a ba yuon jaa bɔɔrlo bonsɩ anyãna ma tɩɛrɛ ba naa a ba yeldɛbɛ,
58010004	bojũu a nadai nɩ a bʋʋr jɩ̃ɩ maa tʋɔrɔ ire a yeldɛbɛ bara ɛ.
58010005	A lɛ jũu, a Kɩrɩsɩto na waara ka a wɛr pɔ, nɩtɔ̃ lɛ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn, "A bɔɔrlo bonsɩ nɩ a bʋ̃kʋrsɩ, faa bʋɔraa ɛ, tɩchɛ ɩ̃gãn lɛ fʋ chɔɔr kʋ ma.
58010006	A bɔɔrlo bonsɩ ban chʋnɔ̃ nɩ a ba 'mabfʋ bʋ̃kʋrsɩ, fʋ pʋɔ maa pɛl yaa ɛ.
58010007	Ka n pãa 'yɛr, maa nɩ nyã, nɩtãa lɛ an sɛb a n yele a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ. N Nãaŋmɩn, n wa naa ɩka n wa ɩ a fʋ bɔfʋ."
58010008	Wʋ den nie 'yɛr, "A bɔɔrlo bonsɩ nɩ a kʋfʋsɩ nɩ a dʋ̃n ala ban ma kʋ chʋm nɩ a ba tulo kʋfʋsɩ ala, faa bʋɔraa ɛ, fʋ pʋɔ ba pɛl ɛ," an sɔɔ ɩ ɩka a nɛbinãa lɛ 'yɛr ɩka ba ɩ a lɛ.
58010009	A wʋ pãa 'yɛr, "Maa nɩ nyã, n wa naa ɩka n wa ɩ a fʋ bɔfʋ." Wʋ tɔɔn a 'lɔ na de nie bar, tɩ de a ayi sʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a jie.
58010010	A nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ jũu lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn maal sɩ, a sɩ ɩ nɩsʋ̃n a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na de a wʋ ɩ̃gãn lon a bɔɔr kpo kpo kʋ sɩ.
58010011	A Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrloro, bɩbir jaa lɛ wʋ ma ara tɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ a ba puorfʋ tʋ̃bie. Waa gala a bɔɔr lofʋ nyã na maa tʋ̃ɔ de yelbier bar ɛ.
58010012	Tɩchɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na wa lo a bɔɔr kpo kpo nyã baar a yelbier jũu, wʋ pãa tɩ jɩ̃nɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nũsʋ̃ɔ jie.
58010013	An yi a lɛ daar jaa, wʋ chɛlɛ naa a Nãaŋmɩn na wa de a wʋ dɔ̃dẽme kʋ wʋ a ba lɩɛb a wʋ gbɛɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie,
58010014	bojũu gbɛbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ wʋ lo a bɔɔr, ka a sɛɛ kʋ a bala wʋn maal ka ba ɩ chɛchɛ.
58010015	A Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ mɩ 'yɛr yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa kʋ sɩ nɩ a yele nyã, wʋ den nie 'yɛr,
58010016	"Nyã lɛ ɩ a nɛtɩraa nyã ɩn wa tara nɩ ba, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wa po baar. Lɛ lɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr. Ɩn den a n nɛbinsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba nyãn pɔ, naa sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba tɩɛrsɩ pɔ."
58010017	Na wʋ pãa lɛ 'yɛr pʋɔ, "A ba yelbier nɩ a ba chɛfʋsɩ tʋ̃bie, n kʋ̃ lɛ tɩɛraa go ɛ."
58010018	Nãaŋmɩn na wa vɛ̃ a yelbier anyãna kʋ nɩrɛ, yelbier bɔɔr lofʋ ba lɛ be be go ɛ.
58010019	A lɛ jũu n yɛɛr, sɩn ben tara a 'lafʋ nyã na tɩ kpɛ a Jichɛchɛ Wʋ Jaa Chɛchɛ Jie a Yesu jɩ̃ɩ jũu,
58010020	na wʋ yuo a yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔr nɩbir paalaa na 'mar tu a fɔvaraa 'lɔ pɔ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn,
58010021	na sɩ be tara a bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ nyã na kaara a Nãaŋmɩn yir,
58010022	yɩ ɩ a sɩ tɔɔ gbʋr Nãaŋmɩn nɩ nyãa nyã na vɩɛlɛ, nɩ a sɔɔfʋ na tɩrɛ. Bojũu wʋ mɩr a sɩ nyãn, na wʋ fɩɛl sɩ yin a tɩɛr sɔ̃ɔnaa pɔ, na wʋ pɛɛ a sɩ ɩ̃gãma nɩ a kɔ̃sʋ̃ɔ ala.
58010023	Yɩ vɛ̃ a sɩ nyɔɔ a sɩ tɩɛrtɔfʋ nyã sɩn sɔɔ jaa chɩ̃chɩ̃ tara, bojũu a 'lɔ na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ sɩ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ.
58010024	Yɩ vɛ̃ a sɩ kpãkpãana taa mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir nʋ̃fʋ nɩ vɩla maalfʋ pɔ.
58010025	Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa vɛ̃ ka sɩ ma bara taa sɛ̃ lɔ̃ɔfʋ ɛ, nɩtãa lɛ a bamɩne na ma ɩrɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ vɛ̃ a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn, na sɩ ma maala a lɛ sɔ̃ɔ jaa, an ɩ a Bɩbir tɔɔrɔ na gbʋrɔ.
58010026	Ala ɩ sɩ chɛnɛ na bɔ̃ɔn jaa tɩ ma maala a yelbier sɩn wa bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ baar, yelbier bɔɔrlo bon jaa ba lɛ be be go ɛ,
58010027	tɩchɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ tɛɛ lɛ sɩ chɛlɛ nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ, nɩ a bũu dagel 'lɔ na wa di a Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃dẽme.
58010028	Nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa dɔ̃ɔ tɔr a lɛ a Mosesɩ na 'yɛr bin, ka a nɩbɛ ayi bɩɩ nɩbɛ ata wa di dãasɩɛ ɩka yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ wʋ ɩ a lɛ, ba ma kʋ naa a nɩnyɩnɛ tɩ maa kaa wʋ nɩbaal ɛ.
58010029	Ge buor lɛ yɩ tɩɛr Nãaŋmɩn na ge a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie nyã nɩ gbɛɛ, a nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ na maal fɩka waa ɩ bʋ̃chɛchɛ ɛ, a jɩ̃ɩ nyã na ɩ a nɛtɩraa na maal wʋ a wʋ tor, ka wʋ tʋ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ Sɩɛ?
58010030	Bojũu sɩ bɔ̃ɔn a 'lɔ na 'yɛr, "Maa lɛ so a sãn yaafʋ, ɩn lɩɛb yaa a sãn," wʋ lɛ bɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr go, "A sɩ Soro na tɔɔr a wʋ nɩbɛ 'yɛr."
58010031	A ɩn dãbɩ̃yele, ala ɩ fʋ faan lo a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbir nyã nũu pɔ.
58010032	Yɩ tɩɛr kaa a lɛ daar yɩn dɔ̃ɔ be be, tɩ wa nyɛ a chãa, a lɛ yɩn ba gbɛr tuor a dɔɔyɛ yɔɔ ala.
58010033	Sɔ̃ɔ kɔ̃ɔ, chãa pɔ jaa lɛ ba ma tʋrɔ yɩ na ba gere nɩ yɩ. Daar kɔ̃ɔ, yɩ ma 'mantãan a bala mɩ ban gere a lɛ.
58010034	Yɩ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ tara nɩbaal nɩ a bala ban nyɔɔr pɔɔ a die pɔ, na yɩ mɩ tara pʋpɛl an ba bã yɩ ɛ, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban fa a yɩ bʋ̃tarsɩ, bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka yɩ mɩ̃ɛ tara naa bʋ̃tarsɩ na ɩ gar a anyãna na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
58010035	A lɛ jũu, yɩ taa lɔb a tɩɛr sʋ̃ nyã bar ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn na yab yɩn gar a lɛ.
58010036	Yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir tara kãnyir na yɩ maala a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ, yɩn wa nyɛn a lɛ wʋn tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ.
58010037	Bojũu a chɛn bɩ̃lãa ka a, "'Lɔ na waara, wʋn wa naa. Wʋ kʋ̃ kor ɛ.
58010038	Tɩchɛ a maa torfʋ sʋɔ 'lɔ, na kpɩɛrɛ naa nɩ sɔɔfʋ. 'Lɔ wa lɩɛb puor 'lɔ, n pʋɔ kʋ̃ pɛl wʋ ɛ."
58010039	Tɩchɛ sɩn ba ɩ a bala na lɩɛrɛ a puor sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩ ɩn a bala na sɔɔ de, na sɩ nyɛ faafʋ.
58011001	Pʋ̃pãanyã, a sɔɔfʋ nyã vɛ̃ naa ka saa 'lɔɔrɔ gbɛr ɛ, yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa a bon 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩn tara a tɩɛr tɩ ba nyɛn nɩbir ɛ.
58011002	A sɔɔfʋ nyã lɛ a kõr dẽme dɔ̃ɔ tara, ka a Nãaŋmɩn dãn ba.
58011003	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ a ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɩka Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ɔ de a wʋ nɛɛ 'yɛrbie maal a tẽe, nɩ a saaju wʋ jaa, ka a bonsɩ sɩn ben nyɛrɛ, a ba ɩ a dɔ̃ɔ be be ka wʋ de maal ɛ.
58011004	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Abel bɔɔrlo bonsɩ wʋn de kʋ Nãaŋmɩn ɩ gar a Kain bɔɔrlo bonsɩ. Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Nãaŋmɩn dãn wʋ 'yɛr ɩka a wʋ yele tor naa, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a Abel kʋfʋsɩ nyã 'yɛr, wʋn sɔɔ kpi gba, tɩchɛ a sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃n ka wʋ chɛnɛ 'yɛrɛ.
58011005	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka Nãaŋmɩn wa de a Enok bʋ̃nɩbir. 'Lɔ ba kpi bɔ̃ɔ kũu ɛ, baa lɛ wa nyɛ wʋ jaa go ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ wa de wʋ. Bojũu sɛrɛ tɩchɛ ka wʋ wa chen, Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr a ɩka a Enok yele nʋ̃mɔ̃ wʋ naa.
58011006	Nɩrɛ ba wa tara sɔɔfʋ ɛ, an ɩn tuo wʋn na tʋ̃ɔ pɛl Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ, bojũu nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa waara a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, wʋ sɔɔn ɩka wʋ ben be, na wʋ mɩ ma yara a bala na mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir bʋɔrɔ wʋ.
58011007	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Nowa tu a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ tɩ ba nyɛn nɩbir ɛ, tɩ na wʋ de dãbɩ̃ɛ maal a daka bulomtum faan a wʋ yir dẽme nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ. A wʋ sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃ naa ka wʋ 'yɛr nɛtuo 'yɔ̃ɔ a wɛr nɩbɛ ba jaa ban tɔr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr jũu, tɩ na wʋ lɩɛb a yeltorsɩ bʋ̃dire a wʋ sɔɔfʋ jũu.
58011008	Abraham sɔɔfʋ jũu, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ bʋɔl wʋ ɩka wʋ yi chen a jie 'lɔ na wa ɩ a wʋ sofʋ daar kɔ̃ɔ, wʋ tu naa a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ na wʋ chen, wʋn gba na ba bɔ̃ɔ a jie wʋn chiine ɛ.
58011009	Sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃ naa ka wʋ tɩ kpɩɛrɛ a nɛtɩraa tẽe 'lɔ pɔ ɩ sãan a be a paal 'lɔ pɔ. A gãma sɛɛr ala pɔ lɛ wʋ dɔ̃ɔ 'mataa kpɩɛrɛ nɩ a Isaakɩ nɩ a Jekɔb, na ba mɩ pʋɔ wʋ na wa so a jie 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a wʋ nɛɛ.
58011010	Bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ kaara niem ɩka wʋ nyɛ yir par ban sʋ̃ɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ ɩ a mɩmɩɛrɛ.
58011011	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Abraham na dɔ̃ɔ kor ɩ danyɔ̃ɔ, ka a wʋ pɔɔ Saara mɩ ab, tɩ ba chɛnɛ na dɔɔ bie. Wʋ tara na sɔɔfʋ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ wʋn tɩr kʋ wʋ.
58011012	Ka a dabʋ̃'yen nyã na kor bʋ̃tul ta kũu, tɩ wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔn par ka ba waa fɩka a ŋmɛrbie na be a saaju, na ba kaara man nɛɛ bire kaar fʋn kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ sɔr ɛ.
58011013	A nɩbɛ banyãna sɔɔn Nãaŋmɩn tɩ tãn a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban kpi. Baa nyɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ ba ɛ, nɩdaa lɛ ba gbã nyãa tɩ sɔɔ de, na ba sɔɔ ɩka sãanba nɩ nɩyʋɔrsɩ lɛ ba ɩ ka a wɛr pɔ.
58011014	A nɩbɛ banyãna na 'yɛr a anyãna, wiil ɩka ba kaara na bʋɔrɔ a tẽe 'lɔ na ɩ a ba mɩ̃ɛ tʋɔr.
58011015	Ala ɩ ba dɔ̃ɔ tɩɛrɛ a paal 'lɔ ban yi, ban taa tʋ̃ɔn lɛ lɩɛb kul a be.
58011016	Tɩ lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, ba dɔ̃ɔ tɩɛrɛ a paal 'lɔ na gar a be, na be a saaju. Ala lɛ so ka a vɩ̃ ba kʋrɔ wʋ wʋn ɩ a ba Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, bojũu wʋ chɔɔr a tẽe kʋ ba.
58011017	Sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃ naa ka Abraham, a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na bɛɛr wʋ kaa ka wʋ sɔɔ de a wʋ bidaba Isaakɩ ka wʋ ɩ a bɔɔrlo bon a wʋn lon a bɔɔr. 'Lɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ de a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ wʋ, tɩ na wʋ sɔɔ de a wʋ bidabʋ̃'yen tɛɛ nyã na lon a bɔɔr.
58011018	Nãaŋmɩn gba na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ ɩka, "Isaakɩ lɛ na 'yɔ̃ɔ a fʋ par, lɛ ɩn tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ fʋ."
58011019	Abraham tɩɛr bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na tʋ̃ɔn sɩ̃ɩ kũu, ka a nyɛtãan fɩka wʋ nyɛn a Isaakɩ na yi a kũu pɔ.
58011020	Sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃ naa ka Isaakɩ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ Jekɔb nɩ a Esau a ba nɩdaar kɔ̃ɔ yele.
58011021	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Jekɔb na ta a kũu, wʋ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ a Josefʋ bibiir ba jaa tɩ na wʋ guun lan a wʋ dãgbal diiraa tɩ puor Nãaŋmɩn yãan.
58011022	Sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃ naa ka a Josefʋ kũu na wa gbʋrɔ, tɩ wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a Isɩral nɩbɛ a Ijipitɩ tẽe pɔ yifʋ 'yɛr kʋ ba, na wʋ man ba a lɛ ban na ɩ nɩ a wʋ kɔbɔ.
58011023	Sɔɔfʋ nyã vɛ̃ naa ka a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban dɔɔ a Mosesɩ a wʋ dɔɔrbɔ sɔɔl wʋn bar ŋmɛrsɩ ata. Bojũu ba nyɛn wʋn ɩ bivɩla, na baa joro a nãa binfʋ ɛ.
58011024	Sɔɔfʋ nyã vɛ̃n a lɛ a Mosesɩ na wa nʋ̃ɔ, waa sɔɔ ka ba bʋɔlɔ wʋ a nãkpɛ̃ɛ Faaro bipɔɔ bie ɛ.
58011025	Wʋ kãan ir ban na 'mataa gen wʋ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ gar wʋn na di a yelbier nʋ̃ɔ bɩ̃lãa tɛɛ.
58011026	Wʋ nyɛn wʋn na di dɔɔyɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto jũu ka a tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ gar a Ijipitɩ tẽe pɔ nãbomo. Bojũu daar kɔ̃ɔ sãyar lɛ wʋ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir kaara.
58011027	Sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃ naa ka a Mosesɩ yi be a Ijipitɩ tẽe pɔ, tɩ ba joro a nãa suur ɛ. Wʋ tara na kãnyir, bojũu wʋ nyɛn a 'lɔ a nɩbir na maa nyɛ ɛ.
58011028	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ wʋ de tun a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛr a Gõl Bar Bɩbir 'yɛr, na wʋ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ ka ba bol a jɩ̃ɩ a ba dɔ̃dɔ̃ ɛ, ka a sɔ̃ɔfʋ 'lɔ na waara ba tʋ̃ɔ sɩɩr a Isɩral nɩbɛ bidadɔ̃n ɛ.
58011029	Sɔɔfʋ vɛ̃ naa ka a Man Jɩɛ var lɩɛb sɔr, ka a Ijipitɩ dẽme mɩ na wa ta nyɛ a lɛ na ba kpɛ ka a man di ba jaa.
58011030	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ vɛ̃ ka a Jeriko dachin kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ wʋ jaa gel lo, a lɛ a Isɩral nɩbɛ na wa gʋɔr a tẽe wʋ jaa a ber ayopõi tuor.
58011031	Sɔɔfʋ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ faa a sɛ̃sɛ̃ pɔɔ 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Worahab, bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ de a bala ban tʋ̃ ɩka ba tɩ jʋʋr a tẽe kaa. Waa dɔ̃ɔ pʋɔ a bawõnsɩ pɔ kpi ɛ.
58011032	N lɛ man bo go? N ba tara jaa na man lɛ a Gɩdɩyɔn nɩ Barakɩ nɩ Samson nɩ Jefeta nɩ a Nãa David nɩ Samuwɛl nɩ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na tʋ̃ 'yɛr ɛ,
58011033	bala lɛ de sɔɔfʋ jɛb na ba tʋ̃ɔn nãmɩne, tɩ maal a lɛ na sɛɛ, nyɛn a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ. Bala lɛ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ kpal a jubɛrɛ nɛɛr,
58011034	na ba kpĩin a bũu dagel, tɩ na ba jo faa a ba mɩ̃ɛ a sɔbɛrɛ ala ban taa kʋn ba. Bala lɛ dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a nɩbaalsɩ, na ba lɩɛb nɩkpɩ̃ɛn, na ba lɩɛb gãdaar a jɛɛr pɔ tʋ̃ɔ a ba dɔ̃dẽme.
58011035	Pɔbɔ mɩ lɛ nyɛn a ba nɩbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ kpi tɩ lɛ lɩɛb ir ɩ vʋɛ. Ba gen bamɩne putuger. Bala ta sɔɔ, ba kʋ̃ naa ge ba ɛ, tɩ ba tɔr tɩ chɛnɛ ara a ba sɔɔfʋ bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba wa nyɛ a kũu 'lɔ pɔ irfʋ na ɩ gar a nyã.
58011036	Ba lan bamɩne na ba fɔb ba, tɩ lũn bamɩne mɩ nɩ bɔ̃jɔrsɩ tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ pɔɔfʋ die pɔ.
58011037	Ba lɔb bamɩne nɩ kusɩbɛ kʋ, tɩ ma chɛ bamɩne mɩ var a yi, tɩ kʋn bamɩne mɩ naa sʋɔ. Piir gãma nɩ bʋʋr gãkpoor lɛ bamɩne mɩ ma dɔ̃ɔ su yʋɔrɔ nɩ na ba ɩ nɔ̃n dẽme, ka ba tara ba gere tɩ sɩlɛ ba a pɔrɔ jaa a lɛ nɛ.
58011038	Ka a wɛr nyã ba ta sɛɛ ɩka wʋ tara a nɩbɛ banyãna ɛ, ka ba bãra yʋɔrɔ be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ nɩ a tɔ̃n jur, kpɩɛrɛ a tɔ̃n bɔɔr pɔ nɩ a tũlotuursɩ bɔɔr ala ban ya a tẽe.
58011039	A nɩbɛ banyãna ba jaa nyɛn dãasɩvɩla a ba sɔɔfʋ jũu, tɩchɛ a bonsɩ ala a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ tɩr a nɛɛ ba ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba nyãa ɛ.
58011040	Nãaŋmɩn guor yelvɩɛl na gar a anyã na wʋ gun sɩ, ka wʋ na de sɩ 'matãan ba maal yele a jaa ka a jɩ̃taa.
58012001	A lɛ jũu, a nɩyɔɔ banyãna na ŋmaa jil sɩ a julõjuur kaar dire a dãasɩɛ, yɩ ɩ a sɩ lɔb bon jaa na ŋmaa sɩ sɔr bar nɩ a yelbier ala na maa yaara tɩ bãr sɩ lɔb ɛ, tɩ na sɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir joro nɩ kãnyir tɩ ta a jie ban tʋ̃ɔ gun sɩ.
58012002	Yɩ ɩ a sɩ fur a sɩ nɩbie 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yesu na sɩ kaara wʋ jaa tɩ̃ɩɩ. 'Lɔ lɛ de a nie be a sɩ sɔɔfʋ sɔr pɔ, tɩ baar. 'Lɔ lɛ a pʋpɛl 'lɔ na be a wʋ niem, wʋ din kãnyir kpi be a daa ju, na wʋ sɔɔ a vɩ̃. Wʋ pãa tɩ jɛ̃n be a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ a nũsʋ̃ɔ jie.
58012003	Yɩ tɩɛr a wʋ yele a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ tara a kãnyir, nɩ a lɛ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ jɛɛrɛ nɩ wʋ, yɩ tɩɛr a lɛ, ka a yɩ ɩ̃gãma taa sal a yɩ tɩɛr sɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
58012004	A yɩ mɔ̃fʋ pɔ, yɩn jɛɛrɛ nɩ a yelbier, yaa jɛb ta a jie 'lɔ sɛrɛ a yɩ jɩ̃ɩ na yi ɛ.
58012005	Yɩ ta ĩin a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ a ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn nɩtãa a wʋ bibiir ɛ, "N bie, ta de dekpele 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro kpãafʋ pɔ ɛ, na fʋ ta vɛ̃ ka a fʋ pʋɔ sɔ̃ɔ a lɛ wʋn gɔ̃nɔ̃ fʋ ɛ,
58012006	bojũu a sɩ Soro ma kpãana na a bala wʋn nʋ̃, na wʋ ma tɔɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa toor wʋn sɔɔ de maal a wʋ bie."
58012007	Yɩ tara kãnyir a kpãafʋ nyã pɔ. Nãaŋmɩn maala yɩ naa a wʋ bibiir. Bojũu bibuor lɛ be be, ka a wʋ sãa maa tɔɔ wʋ toor ɛ?
58012008	Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa ba wa nyɛ a toor tɔɔfʋ a wʋ bibiir kaar ɛ, ka lɛ sãa yir bibiir lɛ ba ɩ.
58012009	Sɩ jaa lɛ tara a sãamɩne ka ba ma kpãa sɩ, tɩ sɩ chɛnɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba. Ŋmɩnɛ lɛ a sɩ kʋ̃ pãa siir sɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a 'lɔ na ɩ a sɩ sɩɩr nɩ a nyɛvʋr Sãa gar a lɛ ɛ!
58012010	A sɩ sãamɩne ma kpãa sɩn jaa bɩ̃lãa tun a lɛ ban tɩɛr ɩka a ɩ naa. Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn ma kpãa sɩ naa, ka sɩ ɩ nɩsʋ̃n, a sɩn nɩ 'lɔ 'mataa põ a wʋ chɛchɛ.
58012011	Kpãafʋ ba be be na ɩ nʋ̃ɔ a pielfʋ daar ɛ, tɩchɛ a ma ɩn tuo. A puor lɛ a ma pãa wɔ̃ torfʋ, nɩ nyã'maar kʋ a bala na sɔɔ tu.
58012012	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ir ɩ̃gãn sal yin a yɩ nuur nɩ a yɩ gbɛɛ pɔ bar,
58012013	"Tɩ na yɩ chɔɔr a sɔr a wʋ jaa jɩ̃taa a yɩ tufʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ," ka a gbɛrsɩ sa na ba tʋ̃ɔ chiine.
58012014	Yɩ mɔ̃ lɛ jaa yɩn na tʋ̃ɔ ɩ, ka yɩn nɩ nɩrɛ jaa kpɩɛrɛ nɩ nyã'maar, na yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ. Nɩrɛ ba wa ɩ chɛchɛ ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ nyɛ a sɩ Soro ɛ.
58012015	Yɩ kaara sʋ̃, ka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa vɩɛ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ bar ɛ, bɩɩ ka a nyɩɩr tuo kɔ̃ɔ taa tɔ yi na wʋ dam yele 'yɔ̃ɔ nɩbɛ ka a ba yɔɔ jie taa sɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
58012016	Yɩ kaara ka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa ɩ sɛ̃sɛ̃yele ɛ, bɩɩ kaara fɩka a Esau na ba dɔ̃ɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɛ, na wʋ de a wʋ kpɛ̃ɛ ɩfʋ nɩ a wʋ difʋ jie tɛɛn bʋ̃diraa gbɛbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ na wʋ di.
58012017	A ala puor, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka wʋ lɛ wa bʋɔrɔ naa a wʋ difʋ jie, ka a sãa tɔr wʋ bar, a wʋ mɩ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ lɩɛb go ɛ. Wʋ gba wa kõn nɩbikʋ̃ɔ nɩ a yele nyã, tɩ waa lɛ nyɛ a sʋ̃ʋfʋ go ɛ.
58012018	Yɩn 'lɔ ba wa a tɔ̃ɔ nyã par yɩn na tʋ̃ɔ sɩɩr ɛ, a 'lɔ na ma dɔ̃ɔ lɩrɛ a bũu, bɩɩ ka a jie ma sɔb lii ka a sajakpuro furo,
58012019	bɩɩ ka ɩlɛ pɛɛlɛ 'yɛrɛ nɩ a nɩrɛ kɔkɔr, bɩɩ ban wõ a kɔkɔr nyã, ba sʋɔr naa ɩka a 'yɛrbie a ta lɛ 'yɛr go ɛ.
58012020	Bojũu baa dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ tara a lɛ a 'yɛr na kpãkpãana ba 'yɛrɛ ɩka, "Ala ɩ dʋ̃ɔ gba wa sɩɩr a tɔ̃ɔ, ba lɔb wʋ nɩ kʋsɩbɛ kʋ."
58012021	Ka a jie dɔ̃ɔ ɩrɛ dãbɩ̃ɛ wʋ jaa, ka Mosesɩ wa tɩ 'yɛr, "N mɩrɛ naa nɩ dãbɩ̃ɛ."
58012022	Tɩchɛ, yɩn 'lɔ wa naa a Jiyon Tɔ̃ɔ par na ɩ a saaju Jerusalɛm, be lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbir nyã kpɩɛrɛ. Yɩ wa lɔ̃ɔn naa a malakasɩ turo turo na lɔ̃ɔ taa nɩ pʋpɛl,
58012023	nɩ a pupuorbiir bala na ɩ a bidɔ̃ɔ, bala yoe lɛ sɛb a be a saaju. Yɩn wa naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'lɔ na tɔɔr a nɩbɛ ba jaa 'yɛr sɛ̃, nɩ a 'lɔ na maal a torfʋ dẽme sɩɩr ka a ɩ chɛchɛ,
58012024	nɩ a Yesu na ɩ a nɛtɩr paalaa nyã 'ma'maala na mɩr a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ ka a 'yɛrɛ naa gar a Abel tʋɔr.
58012025	Yɩ kaara sʋ̃ na yɩ taa tɔr a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛrɛ ɛ. Ala ɩ a bala wʋn dɔ̃ɔ kpãa faa ka a wɛr pɔ ba chɩ̃ɛ ɛ, ŋmɩnɛ an kaara kʋ a sɩn, ala ɩ sɩ lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na kpãana sɩ yire a saaju?
58012026	A sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn kɔkɔr dam a tẽe wʋ jaa, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã 'lɔ wʋ tɩr nɛɛ ɩka, "Daar kɔ̃ɔ go, a ba ɩ a tẽe lɛ ɩn dam ɛ, tɩchɛ ɩn dam a saaju wʋ jaa."
58012027	A 'yɛrbir nyã wʋn 'yɛr ɩka, daar kɔ̃ɔ go, a par lɛ ɩka wʋn ir a bonsɩ ala na ɩ a bʋ̃maalsɩ na dam bar, tɩchɛ a ala na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ dam ɛ, ka ala ara.
58012028	A lɛ jũu, sɩn na ben tara a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nyã na ba tara damfʋ ɛ, yɩ vɛ̃ ka a nʋ̃mɔ̃ sɩ, a sɩ dãna Nãaŋmɩn lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ dãbɩ̃ɛ,
58012029	bojũu a sɩ "Nãaŋmɩn nyã ɩn bũu na dire."
58013001	Yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir na yɩ nʋ̃nɔ̃ taa nɩtãa yɛɛr.
58013002	Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa ĩin sãanba defʋ bar ɛ, bojũu nɩbɛ bamɩne dɔ̃ɔ de sãanba maal ba vɩla, tɩ baa bɔ̃ɔn ɩka malakasɩ lɛ ɛ.
58013003	Yɩ tɩɛr a bala ban nyɔɔr pɔɔ a die pɔ fɩka yɩ mɩ pʋɔ ban be a pɔɔfʋ jie, nɩ a bala ban gere fɩka yɩ mɩ pʋɔ ban dire a dɔɔyɛ.
58013004	Yɩ jaa, yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a kultaa, ka a yɩ gaa jie taa tara chɛfʋ ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn na tɔɔr a bala jaa na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a kultaa nɩ a sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ 'yɛr.
58013005	Yɩ tɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin a libie nʋ̃fʋ pɔ, na yɩ vɛ̃ ka a bɩ̃lãa jaa yɩn tara sɛɛn yi, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa a wʋ gãn pɔ ɩka, "N kʋ̃ wa bar fʋ jaa ɛ, n kʋ̃ wa tɔr fʋ jaa bar ɛ."
58013006	Ka a sɩ pãa na 'la 'yɛr ɩka, "A n Soro lɛ ɩ a n sʋ̃nɔ̃, ka n kʋ̃ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Bo lɛ nɩrɛ na ɩ ma?"
58013007	Yɩ tɩɛrtɔ a yɩ nɩdierbe na dɔ̃ɔ man a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr kʋ yɩ. Yɩ tɩɛr a lɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ be tɩ na yɩ jãn a ba sɔɔfʋ.
58013008	Lɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na be a jãa, lɛ lɛ wʋ chɛnɛ a dɩna na wʋn chɛnɛ a lɛ nɛ bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa.
58013009	Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa vɛ̃ ka a wiil sãan jaa wa tɔɔ yɩ yin ka yɩ tɩ bɔr ɛ, a vɩɛlɛ naa kaa sɩ nyãa nyɛ kpɛ̃ɔ yi a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ pɔ, ka a ta ɩ a bʋ̃diir difʋ na ba tara tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ a bala na dire yaa ɛ.
58013010	Tɩchɛ sɩn tara na a bɔɔr lofʋ jie, be a Juu nɩbɛ bɔɔrlorbo bala na tʋ̃nɔ̃ a be ba tara sɔr na di ɛ.
58013011	A ba bɔɔrlo nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ma den a dʋ̃n ala jɩ̃ɩ kpɛ̃n be a dinie sʋɔ na ɩ a Chɛchɛ Wʋ Jaa Chɛchɛ Jie ka a tɩ ɩ a yelbier vɛ̃ kʋfʋ bon, tɩchɛ ka ba de a nʋ̃nɔ̃ yin a tẽe dãpuor tɩ chʋm bar kaa di.
58013012	Lɛ mɩ lɛ a Yesu di a dɔɔyɛ a tẽe yõo dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ, ka a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ maal a wʋ nɩbɛ ka ba ɩ chɛchɛ.
58013013	Yɩ mɩ ɩ a sɩ yi tɩ pʋɔ wʋ be a yõo na sɩ di a vɩ̃ 'lɔ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ di.
58013014	Bojũu a tẽe nyã sɩn kpɩɛrɛ kʋ̃ kor ɛ, tɩchɛ a sɩ kaara a tẽe 'lɔ na wa.
58013015	Tu a Yesu nyã jie, a lɛ jũu yɩ ɩ a sɩ ma pʋrɔ a wʋ yuor na ɩ pɛɛfʋ ma yire a sɩ nɛgãma pɔ, naa ɩ bɔɔrlo bonsɩ kʋrɔ Nãaŋmɩn.
58013016	Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa ĩin a vɩla maalfʋ bar ɛ, na yɩ ma lɔ̃ɔ põn a yɩ taaba, bojũu a bɔɔrlo bonsɩ anyãna lɛ pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ.
58013017	Yɩ turo a yɩ nɩdierbe nɛɛ, na yɩ siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ ba. Bala lɛ kaara yɩ, na ban wa man a yɩ yele kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn. Yɩ turo a ba nɛɛ ka a ba tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɩ nʋ̃ɔ naa ta ɩ tuor kʋ ba ɛ, naa ta mɩ ɩ pɔrɔ a yɩ sɛ̃ ɛ.
58013018	Yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ sɩ, sɩn sɔɔ naa ɩka yele jaa ba be a sɩ tɩɛr pɔ ɛ, a sɩ bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka sɩ kpɩɛrɛ a lɛ na tor sɔr jaa pɔ.
58013019	Maa 'lɔ, n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa ɩka yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn kʋrɔ ma ka n nyɛ sɔr naa tʋ̃ɔ lɩɛb fɔɔ tɩ a yɩ sɛ̃.
58013020	A Nãaŋmɩn nyã'maar sʋɔ na tu a jɩ̃ɩ ala wʋn de tɩr a nɛtɩraa na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, na wʋ sɩ̃ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto a kũu pɔ, 'lɔ na ɩ a pɛchiin gbɔɔraa,
58013021	wʋ sʋ̃ʋ yɩ nɩ vɩla jaa bʋrɔ ka yɩ tʋ̃ɔ maal a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ, na wʋ mɩ tũ a sɩ pɔ a lɛ na pɛlɛ a wʋ pʋɔ tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto. 'Lɔ lɛ so a tɩɩr bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
58013022	N yɛɛr, n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa ɩka yɩ tu a n kpãafʋ 'yɛrbie anyãna, bojũu a 'yɛrbie anyã ɩn sɛb ba ɩ yɔɔ ɛ.
58013023	N bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka ba yuon a sɩ yɛbɛ Timoti bar, 'lɔ wa tɔ̃ɔ ta fɔɔ, ɩn tara wʋn 'mataa tɩn ka yɩ tɩ nyɛ wʋ.
58013024	Yɩ puor a yɩ nɩdierbe ba jaa nɩ a pupuorbiir ba jaa jaa. Bala mɩ na yi a Itali mɩ puoro yɩ naa.
58013025	A wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋ be a yɩ jaa sɛ̃.
59001001	Jemesɩ, na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto gbãgbaa, puoro naa a Isɩral bala pie nɩ ayi na yaar a wɛr wʋ jaa.
59001002	N yɛɛr, yɩ tara pʋpɛl, ala sɔɔ ɩ yelyɔɔ wõnõ yɩ naa.
59001003	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka yɩn jãn naa tara kãnyir a yɩ bɛɛr kaa sɔ̃ɔ.
59001004	Yɩn jãn tʋ̃ɔ tara kãnyir, a lɛ na vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ tʋ̃ɔ baa, tɩ na yɩ taa wa faa bon jaa ɛ.
59001005	Ala ɩ yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa bʋɔrɔ naa yɛ̃, wʋ sʋɔr yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ na kʋrɔ nɩrɛ jaa pɔrɔ, wʋ ɩn nɩmɩ̃ɛ, wʋ kʋ̃ mɔ̃ɔ fʋ ɛ.
59001006	Tɩchɛ yɩn wa sʋɔr bon jaa, yɩ tara sɔɔfʋ na yɩ ta baala ɛ. Nɩrɛ jaa na baala kaara nɩtãa man kʋ̃ɔ sɛsɛbɛ na furo dãdaala.
59001007	Ala ɩ fʋ ɩ naa a nɩrɛ nyã tɔ sʋɔ, ta tɩɛr ɩka, fʋn nyɛn bon jaa yi a sɩ Soro sɛ̃ ɛ.
59001008	A nɩrɛ na tara tɩɛr ayi, wʋ maa ba gbɛr ara yele jaa pɔ wʋn ɩrɛ ɛ.
59001009	Nãaŋmɩn puoro nɔ̃ɔsʋɔ wʋ chɩlɛ, bojũu wʋ do naa.
59001010	Tɩchɛ a taraa sʋɔ mɩ wʋ chɩlɛ a wʋ suufʋ pɔ, bojũu wʋn suor naa fɩka mɔpuul.
59001011	Bojũu a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ ma nyãa naa ka a tʋl ŋme ka a ko suor, a vapuul ma suor naa ka a vɩla baar. Lɛ lɛ a taraa sʋɔ kaara, 'lɔ wa tʋ̃nɔ̃ a wʋ yar tʋ̃mɔ̃.
59001012	Pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ na di kãnyir ara a bɛɛr kaa pɔ, tɩ na waa lo ɛ. Bojũu a nɩrɛ 'lɔ lɛ na nyɛ a nyɛvʋr nãa jupil 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a bala na nʋ̃ wʋ.
59001013	Bɛɛr kaa wa wa nɩrɛ sɛ̃, wʋ ta 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ bɛɛr wʋ kaa ɛ. Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ de bier bɛɛr nɩrɛ kaa ɛ, a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ ba bɛɛrɛ nɩrɛ kaara ɛ.
59001014	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa yelbier vɔlaa lɛ ma bɛɛr wʋ kaa na a nyɔɔ wʋ.
59001015	A vɔlaa anyãna lɛ na tara pʋɔ naa dɔɔ bier, ka a bier nʋ̃ɔ dɔɔ kũu.
59001016	N yɛɛr nʋ̃nʋ̃nbɔ, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka ba bɛl yɩ ɛ.
59001017	Bʋ̃vɩla nɩ kʋfʋ vɩla jaa yire naa a chãa Sãa na be a saaju sɛ̃. Libe ba be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, waa lɩɛrɛ ɛ.
59001018	An wa ta a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ, wʋ dɔɔ sɩn nɩ a wʋ yelmɩ̃ɛ 'yɛr ka sɩ ɩ birdɔ̃ɔ a bʋ̃maalsɩ a jaa pɔ.
59001019	N yɛɛr nʋ̃nʋ̃nbɔ, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a anyãna yɩ ma chɛlɛ fɔfɔɔ tɩ na yɩ ta ma 'yɛrɛ fɔfɔɔ ɛ, bɩɩ nyɛrɛ suur fɔfɔɔ ɛ.
59001020	Bojũu nɩrɛ wa nyɛ suur, wʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ maal yelvɩla ala a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ ɩka a ɩ ɛ.
59001021	A lɛ juu, yɩ bar yele jaa na ɩ dɛɛr bɩɩ bier, tɩ na yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ de a 'yɛrbir 'lɔ na bʋr a yɩ nyãa pɔ, ala lɛ na faa a yɩ sɩɩr.
59001022	Yɩ ta bɛlɛ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a 'yɛr yɩn chɛlɛ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩ yɩ ɩ a 'yɛr mamaalba.
59001023	A nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na wa wõ a 'yɛr tɩ ba sɔɔ de ɛ, wʋ kaara nɩtãa a 'lɔ na chaar a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kaa chãana pɔ,
59001024	wʋn wa yi baar wʋ ĩin a lɛ bar wʋn kaara.
59001025	Tɩchɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir turo a nɛbinãa na ba tara chɛfʋ ɛ, na ma vɛ̃ ka fʋ so a fʋ mɩ̃ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn na sʋ̃ʋ wʋ naa nɩ bon jaa pɔ wʋn maal, ala ɩ wʋ chɛl tɩ sɔɔ, tɩ a ba ɩ wõ tɩ ĩin ɛ.
59001026	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ tɩɛr ɩka wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn puorbo tɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ nyɔɔ a wʋ jãlbir ɛ, wʋ bɛlɛ na wʋ mɩ̃ɛ, ka a wʋ puorfʋ ɩ pɔrɔ.
59001027	Puorfʋ 'lɔ na pɛlɛ a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ na wʋ ɩ chɛchɛ na ba tara dɛɛr ɛ. Sʋ̃nɔ̃ a bala na ɩ a kpɩɩr, nɩ a pɔɔkɔɛ, a ba dɔɔyɛ pɔ, tɩ nyɔɔ fʋ mɩ̃ɛ ka a wɛr ta sɔ̃ɔ fʋ ɛ.
59002001	N yɛɛr, yɩn sɔɔ de a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tɩɩr sʋɔ, yɩ taa turo nɩbɛ nʋ̃nɔ̃ ɛ.
59002002	Ala ɩ nɩbɛ ayi wa kpɛ naa a yɩ lɔ̃ɔfʋ jie, ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ pɩ̃ɛ na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔn sɛlma mʋtʋɔ, tɩchɛ ka a ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ ɩ nɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ su bʋ̃jarsɩ.
59002003	Ka yɩ lɩɛb 'yɛr kʋ a 'lɔ na pɩ̃ɛ, "Jɩ̃nɛ ka a dakɔɔ ju," tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a 'lɔ mɩ na su a bʋ̃jarsɩ, "Ara ka bɩɩ wa jɩ̃nɛ ka a tẽe a n gbɛɛ par."
59002004	Ala ɩ lɛ lɛ, a ba ɩ yɩ turo naa a nɩbɛ bamɩne nʋ̃nɔ̃ na yɩ de tɩɛr dɛɛr tɔɔrɔ nɩ a ba 'yɛr ɛ?
59002005	N yɛɛr yɩ chɛlɛ, Nãaŋmɩn ir a bala a wɛr nɩbɛ na nyɛ ka ba ɩ nɔ̃n dẽme ka ban tara sɔɔfʋ tɩ kpɛ̃n a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ wʋn tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ a bala na nʋ̃ wʋ.
59002006	Tɩchɛ yɩ ma kpɛrɛ na a nɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ. A ba ɩ a taraa dẽme lɛ ma ge yɩ ɛ. A ba ɩ bala lɛ ma nyɔɔ yɩ chiin a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ jie ɛ?
59002007	A ba ɩ bala lɛ sɔ̃ɔ a yovɩla 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ yɩ ɛ?
59002008	Ala ɩ yɩ tu naa a nɛɛ 'lɔ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Fʋ nʋ̃ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ a fʋ kaar," yɩ maal vɩla.
59002009	Tɩchɛ yɩn wa turo nʋ̃nɔ̃, yɩ maal dɛɛr, ka a nɛɛ 'yɛr ɩka yɩ bɔr naa na yɩ ɩ a nɛɛ sɔ̃sɔ̃ɔnbɔ.
59002010	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na turo a nɛɛr a jaa tɩ wa 'mab bʋ̃'yen, wʋ sɔ̃ɔn a jaa.
59002011	A 'lɔ na 'yɛr, "Taa sɛ̃nɛ ɛ," 'lɔ mɩ lɛ 'yɛr, "Taa kʋrɔ nɩrɛ ɛ." Fʋ̃ʋ ba sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩ kʋ nɩrɛ, fʋ sɔ̃ɔn a jaa.
59002012	Yɩ 'yɛrɛ tɩ maala bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Nãaŋmɩn na tɔɔr a yɩ 'yɛr nɩtãa lɛ a nɛɛ 'lɔ na ma vɛ̃ ka nɩrɛ so a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ na 'yɛr.
59002013	Bojũu a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar, fʋ̃ʋ nyã na ba dɔ̃ɔ tara nɩbibaal jofʋ ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ mɩ jo a fʋ nɩbibaal ɛ. Nɩbibaal jofʋ tʋ̃ɔn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ.
59002014	Vɩla buor nɩ nyã n yɛɛr, ala ɩ nɩrɛ 'yɛr naa ɩka wʋ tara na sɔɔfʋ, tɩchɛ ba lɔ̃ɔn tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɛ, a sɔɔfʋ nyã na tʋ̃ɔ faa wʋ ɔ?
59002015	Ala ɩ yɛbɛ ɩn ɩ̃gãn kpãakpol tɩ ba tara bʋ̃diir ɛ,
59002016	ka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ 'yɛr kʋ wʋ, "Chiine nɩ nyã'maar, a ɩ vɩla kʋ fʋ ka fʋ nyɛ di tɩɩ," tɩchɛ na faa sʋ̃ʋ wʋ a ɩ̃gãn bʋ̃bʋɔrsɩ ɛ, bo vɩla lɛ a ɩ?
59002017	A lɛ jũu, sɔɔfʋ ka tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba pʋɔ ɛ, wʋ ɩn bʋ̃kũu.
59002018	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ na 'yɛr naa, "Fʋ̃ʋ tara na sɔɔfʋ ka maa mɩ tara a tʋ̃mɔ̃." Wiil ma a fʋ sɔɔfʋ ka tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba pʋɔ ɛ, tɩ n mɩ wiil fʋ a n sɔɔfʋ nɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃.
59002019	Fʋ sɔɔ naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen tɛɛ lɛ be be. A ɩn vɩla. A sɩdɛbɛ gba mɩ sɔɔn de a lɛ, tɩ na ba mɩ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ.
59002020	Fʋ̃ʋ jɔl nyã, sɔɔfʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ na ba pʋɔ ɛ, faa bɔ̃ɔ ka bʋ̃kũu lɛ ɛ?
59002021	A ba ɩ a sɩ sãakpã Abraham wiil a sɔɔfʋ nɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃, wʋn dɔ̃ɔ de a wʋ bie Isaakɩ ɩka wʋ lon bɔɔr ɛ?
59002022	Faa nyɛ a sɔɔfʋ nɩ a tʋ̃mɔ̃ na 'mataa ɛ, ka a wʋ sɔɔfʋ sɛɛ nɩ a lɛ wʋn tʋ̃.
59002023	Ka a lɛ na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ ɩka, "Abraham sɔɔn de Nãaŋmɩn, ka a lɛ vɛ̃ ka wʋ ɩ nɩtor." Ka Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl wʋ wʋ baraa.
59002024	Yaa nyɛ, nɩrɛ na ɩn nɩtor Nãaŋmɩn niem a lɛ wʋn tʋ̃, a ba ɩ a wʋ sɔɔfʋ tɛɛ ɛ.
59002025	A lɛ nɩ wʋ ju lɛ ba dɔ̃ɔ kaa a sɛ̃sɛ̃ pɔɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Worahab ka wʋ ɩ nɩtor, wʋn dɔ̃ɔ de a tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ wiil ba sɔyuo ka ba lɩɛb kul.
59002026	A lɛ a sɩɛ na ma wa yi a ɩ̃gãn pɔ ka wʋ ɩ bʋ̃kũu, lɛ mɩ lɛ a sɔɔfʋ ka tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba pʋɔ ɛ mɩ ɩ bʋ̃kũu.
59003001	N yɛɛr, yɩ jaa yɩ ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka yɩ ɩ wiwiilbe ɛ, bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a sɩn bala na ɩ a wiwiilbe na nyɛn 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ gar nɩrɛ jaa.
59003002	Sɩ jaa ma maal 'mab. Ala ɩ nɩrɛ jaa ba 'yɛr 'mab ɛ, wʋ ɩn nɩtor na wʋ nyɔɔrɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ.
59003003	Sɩ ma 'yɔ̃ɔn a kur a wiisɩ nɛɛr pɔ, ka a ma tu a sɩ nɛɛr, ka sɩ ma lɩɛb chiin jie jaa sɩn bʋɔrɔ.
59003004	Bɩɩ yɩ kaa a gbor bɛrɛ ala a man kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ a sɛsɛkpɛ̃ɛ na ma furo chiine, tɩchɛ a gbor mɔ̃nɔ̃ ma den a vuur mɔ̃ chiin jie jaa wʋn bʋɔrɔ.
59003005	Lɛ mɩ lɛ a jãlbir na ɩ jaa pʋʋrbile a ɩ̃gãn pɔ tɩ ma fere. Wʋ kaara fɩka bũu bir na lo tuu kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ di wʋ jaa.
59003006	A jãlbir mɩ ɩn bũu na ɩ a wɛr dɛɛr na be a sɩ ɩ̃gãn pɔ na wʋ sɔ̃ɔ a ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa bar, na wʋ chʋmɔ̃ a ɩ̃gãn nɩ a bũu dagel 'lɔ na ba kpĩine ɛ.
59003007	Nɩrɛ ma tʋ̃ɔn guol mɔdʋ̃ɔ jaa bʋrɔ, nɩ lubil jaa bʋrɔ, bʋ̃vuuraa jaa bʋrɔ, nɩ a man pɔ bonsɩ.
59003008	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ maa tʋ̃ɔ a wʋ jãlbir ɛ, wʋ ɩn bʋ̃bier na ba pɛ̃nɛ ɛ, na wʋ mɩ ɩ lɔɔ na kʋrɔ.
59003009	A jãlbir nyã lɛ sɩ ma de pɛɛn a sɩ Sãa na ɩ a sɩ Soro, na sɩ lɛ de ma pɔn 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala a Nãaŋmɩn na mɛ ka ba kaara a wʋ kaar.
59003010	A nɛbʋ̃'yen 'lɔ pɔ lɛ a pɛɛfʋ nɩ pɔ'yɔ̃ɔfʋ ma yire. N yɛɛr a ba tor ɛ.
59003011	Kɔ̃vɩla nɩ kɔ̃dɛɛr na tʋ̃ɔ yire bul bʋ̃'yen pɔ bɩɩ?
59003012	N yɛɛr, kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ na tʋ̃ɔ wɔ̃ dãbɩ̃ɩnãa bɩɩ dãbɩ̃ɩnãa na tʋ̃ɔ wɔ̃ kɔ̃kɔ̃ɔ ɔ? Lɛ mɩ lɛ, kɔ̃vɩla nɩ kɔ̃dɛɛr kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ 'mataar yire bul bʋ̃'yen pɔ ɛ.
59003013	A yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ tara na yɛ̃ nɩ bɔ̃ɔfʋ bɩɩ? Vɛ̃ ka a wiil a wʋ maalfʋ pɔ, nɩ lɛ wʋn siir a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ maala nɩ yɛ̃.
59003014	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a yɩ nyãa pɔ, nyuur dɛɛr nɩ tuo, nɩ yobɔyele ben be, yɩ ta wile yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ŋmara jirsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
59003015	A yɛ̃ nyã bʋrɔ ba yi saaju wa ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ ɩ naa a wɛr nyã yɛ̃ nɩsaal na tara ka wʋ yi a sɩdɛɛr sɛ̃.
59003016	Bojũu jie 'lɔ nyuur, nɩ tuo, nɩ yobɔyele na be, be lɛ guor taa ba be ɛ, ka tʋ̃ dɛɛr jaa bʋrɔ be be.
59003017	Tɩchɛ a yɛ̃ 'lɔ, na yi saaju ɩn chɛchɛ na wʋ tara nyã'maar nʋ̃fʋ, nɩ sʋ̃ʋfʋ, nɩ mɩ̃ɛ siirfʋ, nɩ vɩla maalfʋ, na wʋ joro nɩbaal, na wʋ wɔ̃nɔ̃ bisʋ̃n, na waa ooro ɛ, bɩɩ tara nɛɛr ayi ɛ.
59003018	A bala na ba bʋɔrɔ jɛɛr ɛ, na bʋr nɩ nyã'maar, na ŋman yeltorsɩ.
59004001	Nyɩnɛ lɛ a jɛɛr nɩ nɛchɩrɛ yi be a yɩ chara pɔ? A ba ɩ a yi naa a vɔlaa 'lɔ na be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ jɛɛr ɛ?
59004002	Yɩ ma bʋɔrɔ na bon kɔ̃ɔ tɩ yɩ maa nyɛ ɛ, na yɩ ma kʋrɔ taa. Na yɩ ma tara nyuur nɩ bomo, tɩ na yɩ maa nyãa ɛ, na yɩ pãa tara jɛɛr nɩ nɛchɩrɛ, tɩ maa nyãa ɛ, bojũu yɩ maa sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn ɛ.
59004003	Yɩn wa sʋɔr a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, yɩ maa nyɛ ɛ, bojũu yɩ sʋɔr naa nɩ pʋtɩdɛɛr na de maal a lɛ na pɛl a yɩ pʋɔ.
59004004	Yɩn sɛ̃sɛ̃ nɩbɛ ba nyã, yaa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka nɩrɛ nyã na ɩ a wɛr baraa 'laar Nãaŋmɩn ɛ? Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ŋmaa a wɛr nyã baraa ɩn Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃ sʋɔ.
59004005	Ta baala a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr ɩka, yelmɩ̃ɛ jaa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kaara a Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn de 'yɔ̃ɔ sɩ.
59004006	Tɩchɛ Nãaŋmɩn ma kʋ sɩ naa a wʋ wɩ̃ɛfʋ, ala lɛ so a Nãaŋmɩn gãn na 'yɛr, "Nãaŋmɩn ma tɔr naa bala na bʋɔr yuor, tɩ na wʋ ma wɩ̃ɛ a bala na siir ba mɩ̃ɛ."
59004007	A lɛ jũu, yɩ siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, na yɩ tɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin a sɩdɛɛr sʋɔ sɛ̃, wʋn bar yɩn tɩ jo.
59004008	Yɩ tɔɔ gbʋr Nãaŋmɩn, wʋ mɩ na tɔɔn gbʋr yɩ. Yɩn yelbe-ɩrbɛ, yɩ pɛɛ a yɩ nuur na yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr, yɩn tɩɛr ayi dẽme.
59004009	Yɩ waala, na yɩ tara pʋsɔ̃ɔ, na yɩ kõnõ. Yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ laar lɩɛb kõn, ka a yɩ pʋpɛl lɩɛb pʋsɔ̃ɔ.
59004010	Yɩ siir a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a sɩ Soro niem, wʋn 'mɔɔ yɩn ka yɩ do.
59004011	N yɛɛr, yɩ ta sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa yoe ɛ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ yuor, wʋ tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr, wʋ tɔɔrɔ naa a nɛbinãa 'lɔ 'yɛr. Fʋ̃ʋ wa tɔɔrɔ a nɛbinãa 'yɛr, faa turo a lɛ a nɛbinãa na 'yɛr ɛ, tɩ ɩ a wʋ 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ.
59004012	Nãaŋmɩn lɛ bin a wʋ nɛɛ kʋ sɩ, na wʋ ɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ, 'lɔ lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ faa bɩɩ sɔ̃ɔ bar. Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ mɩ nɩ ana na fʋ tɔɔrɔ a fʋ tɔ sʋɔ 'yɛr?
59004013	Yɩ chɛlɛ, a yɩn bala na ma 'yɛr ɩka, "Dɩna bɩɩ bio sɩn chen tẽkpɛ̃ɛ pɔ tɩ maal yuon, da bomo, da nyɛ libie."
59004014	Yaa bɔ̃ɔ lɛn na ɩ bio ɛ, bo lɛ a yɩ nyɛvʋr? Wʋ kaara fɩka ul na lo tɩ wɛl ajienaa.
59004015	Yɩ ta ma 'yɛr ɩka, "Ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn sɔɔ naa ka sɩ tara nyɛvʋr, sɩn maal nyã bɩɩ anyãna."
59004016	Tɩ lɛ an be nɩ nyã, yɩ bʋɔrɔ na yuor, na yɩ wile yɩ mɩ̃ɛ, ka a mɩ̃ɛ wiilfʋ nyã ɩ yelbier.
59004017	Nɩrɛ jaa na pãa bɔ̃ɔ vɩla tɩ ba maal ɛ, wʋ ɩn bier.
59005001	Yɩ chɛlɛ, yɩn tara dẽme, yɩ kõnõ ŋmiere chɛlsɩ a yele 'lɔ na waara a yɩ ju.
59005002	A yɩ nãbomo pʋ̃ɔ naa, ka yɛlɛ mʋʋ a yɩ fɔɔr.
59005003	A yɩ sɛlma nɩ a libie lon sɔrɔ, ka a ba sɔrɔ lofʋ wiil ɩka an di yɩn bũu kaar. A baarfʋ ta naa, tɩ yɩ chɛnɛ bin a nãbomo.
59005004	Yɩ nyɛ a bala yɩn de ka ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ a yɩ por pɔ, tɩ yɩ mɔ̃ɔ ba a yar ka ba kõnõ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ yɩ, ka a yɩ bʋ̃ŋmarba kõn ta a sɩ Soro na ɩ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ.
59005005	Yɩ din nʋ̃ɔ ka a wɛr pɔ lɛ yɩn bʋɔrɔ. Yɩ guol naa yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a lɛ kʋfʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
59005006	Yɩ ma 'yɔ̃ɔn a bala na tor 'yɛr, na yɩ kʋ ba, tɩ baa maal bon jaa ɛ.
59005007	A lɛ jũu, yɛɛr yɩ tara kãnyir tɩ tãn a sɩ Soro waa daar. Kaa nyɛ a lɛ a kʋɔraa na ma tara kãnyir chɛlɛ nɩ a bonsɩ wɔ̃fʋ daar, na wʋ tara kãnyir chɛlɛ a sadɔ̃ɔ nɩ a sabaaraa.
59005008	Yɩn mɩ, yɩ tara kãnyir na yɩ ara kpɛ̃ɔ, bojũu a sɩ Soro waa gbʋr naa.
59005009	Yɛɛr yɩ ta hũhũnõ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa na yɩ taa nyɛ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ ɛ. A 'yɛr tɔɔrɔ ara naa a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ.
59005010	Yɛɛr, yɩ kaa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ bala na de a sɩ Soro yuor 'yɛr 'yɛr, din dɔɔyɛ tɩ tara kãnyir.
59005011	Ala lɛ so ka sɩ bʋɔlɔ ba bɔɔsʋ̃n dẽme. Yɩ wõn a Job kãnyir wʋn tara na yɩ mɩ nyɛ a lɛ a sɩ Soro na maal kʋ wʋ a baaraa. A sɩ Soro ɩn nɩbaal joro, na wʋ maala vɩla.
59005012	N yɛɛr, ala na chɛ lɛ a anyã, yɩ taa pɔrɔ nɩ saaju ɛ, bɩɩ a tẽe ɛ, bɩɩ bon jaa ɛ, tɩ yɩ vɛ̃ ka yɩ ɔ̃ɔ, ɩ ɔ̃ɔ, ka yɩ kai, mɩ ɩ kai. Ka yɩ taa kpɛ 'yɛr pɔ ɛ.
59005013	Wõm pɔɔn a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ bɩɩ? Wʋ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn. Nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ̃n a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ bɩɩ? Wʋ yiele yiel dãna nɩ Nãaŋmɩn.
59005014	A yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ bɩɛrɛ na bɩɩ? Wʋ bʋɔl a pupuorbiir nɩbɛrɛ ka ba wa jɛ wʋ kãa nɩ a sɩ Soro yuor, na ba sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn kʋ wʋ.
59005015	A Nãaŋmɩn ban sʋɔr nɩ sɔɔfʋ na sa naa nɩnyɩnɛ baal, a sɩ Soro na nyɔɔ wʋ naa ka wʋ ir. Ala ɩ wʋ mɩ maal dɛɛr, Nãaŋmɩn na vɛ̃n kʋ wʋ.
59005016	A lɛ jũu, yɩ 'yɛrɛ a yɩ maal dɛbɛ kʋrɔ taa, na yɩ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ taa, ka wʋ sãana yɩ. Nɩtor Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ tara na kpɛ̃ɔ na maal bon.
59005017	Elaija ɩn nɩrɛ a sɩ kaar, wʋ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn nɩbijɩɛ ɩka saa wʋ ta wa ɛ, ka war ŋmaa yuomo ata nɩ ŋmaa.
59005018	Wʋ lɛ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn go ka a saa wa, ka a bonsɩ bul a tẽe naa wɔ̃.
59005019	N yɛɛr, ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ 'mab naa a yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔr pɔ, ka a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ lɩɛb wʋ waan,
59005020	yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a anyã ɩka, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na lɩɛb yelbe-ɩrɛ yin a wʋ yelbier pɔ, wʋ faa wʋn yin kũu pɔ, na wʋ mɩ pɔɔ yelbebe yɔɔ jaa.
60001001	Maa Pita na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nãa lɛ sɛɛrɛ a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a yɩn a Nãaŋmɩn na chɛl ir a yɩ ɩ sãanba yɛ̃yɛl ka a wɛr pɔ, na yɩ be a Pontus, nɩ Galatiya, nɩ Kapadosiya, nɩ Asɩya, nɩ a Bitiniya.
60001002	A Sãa Nãaŋmɩn den nie bɔ̃ɔ yɩ, ka a wʋ Sɩɛ oo yɩ, a yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ, yɩn wõnõ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto toor jũu, ka wʋ mɩr yɩ a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar na dɔɔlɔ yɩn taa.
60001003	Pɛɛfʋ wʋ ta a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto Sãa! A wʋ nɩbaal bɛrma naa, ka wʋ dɔɔ sɩ dɔɔ paalaa, na wʋ kʋ sɩ tɩɛrtɔ vʋr tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wʋn sɩ̃ɩ a kũu pɔ,
60001004	nɩ a nãbomo ala wʋn bin gun sɩ be a saaju, a ba wɛrɛ ɛ, a ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ, bɩɩ jʋɔlɔ ɛ.
60001005	A tu naa yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn Kpɛ̃ɔ ger pɔɔ yɩ, tɩ tãn a bɩbir baaraa 'lɔ a faafʋ 'lɔ na chɔɔr baar na wa nyɩr.
60001006	A anyãna pɔ lɛ yɩ chɩlɛ yɔɔ jaa, an sɔɔ ɩ ɩka yɩn din dɔɔyɛ bɛɛr kaa bʋrɔ bʋrɔ pɔ.
60001007	A anyãna wa naa ka a yɩ sɔɔfʋ na kpɛ̃mɛ gar a sɛlma na ɩ bʋ̃sɔ̃ɔnãa ban ma dʋʋl bũu pɔ ir a dɛɛr bar. A yɩ sɔɔfʋ na lɩɛb ɩ pɛɛfʋ, nɩ tɩɩr, nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na wa nyɩr.
60001008	Yɩ gba na ba nyɛ wʋ ɛ, tɩ na yɩ nʋ̃ wʋ. Yaa gba nyɛ wʋ a pʋ̃pãanyã ɛ, tɩ sɔɔ wʋ, na yɩ sɛɛn a pʋpɛl tɩɩr 'lɔ nɩrɛ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ man ɛ.
60001009	Bojũu yɩ nyɛrɛ naa a yɩ sɔɔfʋ bon na ɩ a yɩ sɩɩr faafʋ.
60001010	A faafʋ nyã 'yɛr lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a wɩ̃ɛfʋ nyã na wa a yɩ sɛ̃. Ba vɩɛr naa a faafʋ nyã na ba chɛ̃pɛ̃ wʋ jaa nɛ nɛ.
60001011	Ba mʋ̃ɔn nɩbir ɩka ba bɔ̃ɔ a sɔ̃ɔ nɩ a yelsɩ ala a Kɩrɩsɩto Sɩɛ na be a ba sɛ̃ na wile ba, a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr a dɔɔyɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto na di nɩ a tɩɩr ala na turo.
60001012	Nãaŋmɩn wiil naa a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ banyãna ɩka a ba ɩ ba mɩ̃ɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ ba tʋ̃nɔ̃ a lɛ ɛ, tɩ chɛ yɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ. A lɛ ban 'yɛr a nyãna yɩn ben wõnõ a pʋ̃pãanyã a bala na mʋɔlɔ a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ tu a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ wʋn tʋ̃ a wʋ yi a saaju. A malakasɩ mɩ gba ta bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba muul kaa a anyãna.
60001013	A lɛ jũu, yɩ chɔɔr a yɩ tɩɛr gun tʋ̃mɔ̃, na yɩ nyɔɔrɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ. Yɩ de a yɩ tɩɛrtɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a wɩ̃ɛfʋ 'lɔ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na kʋ yɩ a wʋ waa daar.
60001014	Yɩn wõnõ a Nãaŋmɩn toor jũu, yɩ taa lɛ maala a kõro mamaalbie ɛ, a lɛ yɩn ba dɔ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
60001015	Tɩchɛ nɩtãa lɛ a 'lɔ na bʋɔl yɩ na ɩ chɛchɛ, yɩ mɩ ɩ chɛchɛ a yɩ yelmaalsɩ a jaa pɔ.
60001016	Bojũu a sɛb ɩka, "Yɩ ɩ chɛchɛ, bojũu n ɩn chɛchɛ."
60001017	Yɩn ma bʋɔlɔ wʋ a yɩ Sãa, 'lɔ lɛ na tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr, na waa turo ɛ, yɩ kpɩɛrɛ a yɩ kpɛfʋ nɩtãa sãanba, na yɩ joro wʋ dãbɩ̃ɛ.
60001018	Bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a ba ɩ bʋ̃sɔ̃ɔnãa fɩka libir, bɩɩ sɛlma lɛ Nãaŋmɩn de yab den yɩ yin a yɩ sãakpãmɩne yelpɔrsɩ ala na lũ yɩ pɔ ɛ,
60001019	tɩchɛ a ɩ naa a Kɩrɩsɩto jɩ̃ɩ vɩla ala na ɩ a pɛraabile na ba tara chɛfʋ ɛ, bɩɩ jɩ̃nɛ jaa ɛ.
60001020	Nãaŋmɩn ir wʋ naa tɩ wa bɩɛr maal a wɛr, tɩchɛ wʋ vɛ̃n ka wʋ nyɩr a sɔ̃ɔ baaraa a yɩ jũu.
60001021	A wʋ jũu lɛ yɩ sɔɔ de a Nãaŋmɩn na ir wʋ a kũu pɔ na wʋ kʋ wʋ tɩɩr, ka a yɩ sɔɔfʋ nɩ a yɩ tɩɛrtɔ na be a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ.
60001022	Pʋ̃pãanyã yɩn chɔɔr a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yɩn turo a yelmɩ̃ɛ jũu, yɩ nʋ̃nɔ̃ naa a yɛɛr sɩrɛ jaa. Yɩ nʋ̃nɔ̃ taa nɩ a yɩ nyãa wʋ jaa.
60001023	Bojũu yɩ nyɛn dɔɔ paalaa 'lɔ na ba ɩ bʋ̃kpiraa ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋn ben be, na ba tu a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr na ɩ vʋr, na be be bɩbir jaa.
60001024	Bojũu, "Nɩsaal kaara naa fɩka mʋɔr, ka a ba tɩɩr wʋ jaa kaara fɩka a mɔpuul. A mʋɔr wa jʋɔl, a puul mɩ ma suor naa.
60001025	Tɩchɛ a sɩ Soro 'yɛr 'lɔ ben be bɩbir jaa." A 'yɛr nyãna lɛ ba mʋɔl kʋ yɩ.
60002001	A lɛ jũu, yɩ ir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin a yosɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr, bɛlfʋ, nɛɛr ayi tarfʋ, nyuur, nɩ kporfʋ jaa bʋrɔ pɔ.
60002002	Yɩ kaara fɩka bipɩlɛ, na yɩ bʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ka ɩ yɩ vɔlaa a bɩr kaar, a yɩn tʋ̃ɔ nʋ̃ɔ a yɩ faafʋ pɔ,
60002003	bojũu an ɩ yɩ lɛm kaa lɛ a sɩ Soro na nʋ̃mɔ̃.
60002004	An ɩ yɩ wa naa a wʋ sɛ̃ na ɩ a Kʋsɩr vʋr a nɩsaal na tɔr bar, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn ir wʋ a wʋ ɩ bʋ̃sʋ̃,
60002005	yɩn mɩ na ɩ fɩka a kʋsɩvʋɛ a ba mɛn yɩ, nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn yir ka yɩ ɩ a wʋ bɔɔrlo chɛchɛsɩ, na yɩ loro a wʋ bɔɔr wʋn sɔɔ tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
60002006	A sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ ɩka, "Nyɛ, n bin a kʋsɩr be a Jiyon tẽe pɔ, a kʋsɩr vɩla 'lɔ ɩn kaa ir ka wʋ ɩ a kʋsɩr ju, ka nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ de wʋ, vɩ̃ kʋ̃ di wʋ ɛ."
60002007	Pʋ̃pãanyã a yɩn bala na sɔɔ de wʋ, wʋ ɩn kʋsɩr sʋ̃. Tɩchɛ a bala na ba sɔɔ de wʋ ɛ, "A kʋsɩr 'lɔ a mɩmɩɛrbɛ na tɔr bar, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a kʋsɩr ju,"
60002008	na, "Wʋ ɩ a kʋsɩr 'lɔ a nɩbɛ na ŋmiere a gbɛɛ, na wʋ ɩ a pie 'lɔ ban bãra loro." Ba ŋmiere naa ba gbɛɛ bojũu ba tɔr naa a 'yɛr 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na dɔ̃ɔ bin ba.
60002009	Tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ, Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ir yɩ a yɩ ɩ a wʋ bɔɔrlo nãmɩne, na yɩ ɩ nɩchɛchɛsɩ, na yɩ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sofʋ, ka yɩ na pɛɛrɛ wʋ, an ɩ 'lɔ lɛ bʋɔl yɩ yin a libe pɔ waan a wʋ chãa herete pɔ.
60002010	Yaa dɔ̃ɔ ɩ a wʋ nɩbɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã yɩ ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ. Yaa dɔ̃ɔ tara a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbaal ɛ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã yɩ tara wʋ naa.
60002011	N barmɩne, n sʋɔrɔ yɩ naa nɩtãa nɩyʋɔrsɩ nɩ sãanba ka a wɛr pɔ ɩka, yɩ ir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin a ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa na ma jɛɛrɛ nɩ a yɩ sɩɩr.
60002012	Yɩ kpɩɛrɛ vɩla a bala na ba puoro sɛ̃, ban sɔɔ gba kpɛrɛ yɩ ɩka dɛɛr lɛ yɩ maala, bala wa nyɛ a yɩ vɩla maalfʋ ban 'yɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr a wʋ waa bɩbir.
60002013	A sɩ Soro jũu, yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a tʋ̃ɔfʋ dẽme, ala sɔɔ ɩ a nãkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ lɛ,
60002014	bɩɩ a nãbil bala wʋn ir bin a tẽn tẽn ka ba kpãana a bala na maala dɛɛr tɩ pɛɛrɛ a bala mɩ na maala a lɛ na tor.
60002015	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ lɛ ɩka yɩn maala vɩla na yɩ pɔɔ a ba bɔ̃ɔ dẽme na ɩ a jɔlɔ nɛɛr.
60002016	Yɩ kpɩɛrɛ nɩtãa sumɩne, tɩchɛ yɩ taa de a mɩ̃ɛ sofʋ nyã pɔɔn yelbier ɛ, tɩ yɩ kpɩɛrɛ fɩka Nãaŋmɩn gbãgbaar.
60002017	Yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩrɛ jaa na yɩ nʋ̃ a yɩ taa Yesu turbo, na yɩ joro Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ, tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a nãa.
60002018	Gbãgbaar, yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a yɩ tʋ̃nbɔ nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, a ta ɩ a bala na bal nɩbir maala yɩ vɩla tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bala mɩ na kpɛ̃mɛ a nɩbir.
60002019	Bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn na maal vɩla kʋ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara tɩɛr vɩla, na wʋ di dɔɔyɛ na ba tara sɔr ɛ, bojũu wʋ tara na Nãaŋmɩn tɩɛr.
60002020	Tɩchɛ bo lɛ na ɩ a yɩ tɔ̃nɔ̃, ala ɩ ba ŋme yɩ naa yɩn tʋ̃ dɛɛr jũu? Tɩchɛ ala ɩ yɩ din dɔɔyɛ yɩn maal vɩla jũu, an ɩn tɔ̃nɔ̃ kʋ yɩ Nãaŋmɩn niem.
