60002021	A anyãna jũu lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl yɩ, bojũu Kɩrɩsɩto mɩ dɔ̃ɔ di dɔɔyɛ, na wʋ maal wiil yɩ ɩka yɩ turo a wʋ pala.
60002022	"Ka waa dɔ̃ɔ maal dɛɛr jaa ɛ, bɩɩ ka bɛlfʋ yi a wʋ nɛɛ pɔ ɛ."
60002023	A lɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ tʋrɔ wʋ, waa mɩ tʋ yaa a sãn ɛ. A dɔɔyɛ na pɔɔ wʋ, waa jo dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Tɩchɛ wʋ den a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɔɔrɔ a 'yɛr jaa dẽ dẽ.
60002024	A wʋ mɩ̃ɛ lɛ tuo a sɩ yeldɛbɛ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn pɔ a daa ju, ka sɩ mɩ na kpi kʋ yelbier tɩ be be kʋ yeltorsɩ. A wʋ fɛlɛ ala jũu lɛ sãa sɩ.
60002025	Na yɩ kaara fɩka piir na dɔ̃ɔ bɔrɔ, tɩchɛ pʋ̃pãanyã yɩ lɩɛb wa a pɛchinɛ na kaara a yɩ sɩɩr sɛ̃.
60003001	Pɔbɔ, a lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, yɩ sɩɩr yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a yɩ sɩrbɛ. Bamɩne baa sɔɔ puor ɛ, tɩchɛ a yɩ befʋ na tʋ̃ɔn lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr a ba puoro,
60003002	bala wa nyɛ a lɛ a yɩ maalfʋ na ɩ vɩla, nɩ lɛ yɩn 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ.
60003003	Yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a yɩ vɩla ɩ a yõo pɩ̃ɛfʋ tɛɛ ɛ, nɩtãa a ju wobfʋ, sɛlma bɔ̃jɔrsɩ yarfʋ, nɩ a fɔnɩbikpɩ̃ɛn sɛfʋ ɛ.
60003004	Tɩchɛ yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ pɩ̃ɛfʋ be pʋɔm na ba jʋɔlɔ ɛ, na ɩ vɩla, hɛ lɛ lɛ lɛ, nɩ jomm, ala lɛ ɩ vɩla a Nãaŋmɩn niem.
60003005	Bojũu nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃ lɛ a mama pɔɔsʋ̃n bala na tara a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɛr ma maal a ba mɩ̃ɛ vɩla. Na ba sɔɔ turo, na ba sɩɩr ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a ba sɩrbɛ.
60003006	Lɛ mɩ lɛ a Saara na dɔ̃ɔ wõnõ a Abraham toor na wʋ ma bʋɔlɔ wʋ a wʋ soro. Yɩn lɛ ɩ a wʋ bibiir, ala ɩ yɩ maala na a lɛ na vɩɛlɛ na yɩ kʋ̃ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
60003007	Sɩrbɛ a lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, yɩ tɩɛrɛ a yɩ pɔbɔ yɩn lɔ̃ɔ kpɩɛrɛ nɩ. Yɩ kaara ba nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, bojũu baa tara kpɩ̃ɛn jɩ̃ yɩ ɛ, tɩ na ba pʋɔ yɩ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ kʋfʋ 'lɔ na ɩ nyɛvʋr, ka bon jaa taa var a yɩ Nãaŋmɩn sʋɔrfʋ ɛ.
60003008	A 'yɛr baaraa lɛ a anyã, yɩ jaa yɩ tara tɩɛr bʋ̃'yen, na yɩ kaara taa nɩbaal, na yɩ nʋ̃ taa maala vɩla kʋrɔ taa nɩ mɩ̃ɛ siirfʋ.
60003009	Yɩ ta de yelbier yãan yelbier sãn ɛ, bɩɩ tʋbir yãan tʋbir sãn ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ 'yɛr nɛvɩla 'yɔ̃ɔ ba, bojũu a anyã 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔl yɩ ɩka yɩn nyɛn sʋ̃ʋfʋ.
60003010	Bojũu, "Ala ɩ nɩrɛ nʋ̃n nyɛvʋr na wʋ bʋɔrɔ bɩbivɩɛlsɩ wʋ ir wʋ nɛɛ yin 'yɛrdɛɛr nɩ bɛlfʋ pɔ.
60003011	Wʋ lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ yelbier tɩ maala vɩla, na wʋ bʋɔrɔ nyã'maar joro turo a wʋ puor.
60003012	Bojũu a sɩ Soro kaara naa a bala na tor, na wʋ wõnõ a ba sʋɔrfʋ. Tɩchɛ a sɩ Soro pʋɔ ma sɔ̃ɔ naa nɩ a bala na ma maala yelbier."
60003013	An lɛ na ge yɩ ala ɩ yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir maala vɩla?
60003014	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ yɩ gba din dɔɔyɛ yɩn maala vɩla jũu, Nãaŋmɩn na sʋ̃ʋ yɩ naa. "Yɩ ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ nɩ a ba vuurfʋ ɛ. Yɩ taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ,"
60003015	Tɩchɛ a yɩ nyãn pɔ, yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a yɩ Soro. Na yɩ ma chɔɔr sɔ̃ɔ jaa ala ɩ nɩrɛ wa sʋʋr yɩ naa a tɩɛrtɔ 'lɔ yɩn tara, tɩchɛ yɩ ma man naa jomm nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ,
60003016	na yɩ vɛ̃ ka a yɩ tɩɛr chaar, ka a bala na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yɩ yuor yɩn turo a Kɩrɩsɩto jũu, ka vɩ̃ na kpɛ ba, nɩ a ba yosɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr.
60003017	An ɩn vɩla ala ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ lɛ, yɩn di dɔɔyɛ vɩla maalfʋ jũu, gar yɩn na di dɔɔyɛ dɛɛr maalfʋ jũu.
60003018	Bojũu Kɩrɩsɩto kpi naa a yɩ yelbier jũu gbɛbʋ̃'yen tɛɛ, a 'lɔ na tor kʋ a bala na ba tor ɛ, ɩka wʋ waan yɩ Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃. Ba kʋ naa a wʋ ɩ̃gãn, tɩchɛ ka a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ sɩ̃ɩ wʋ a kũu pɔ,
60003019	a Sɩɛ nyã lɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto chiin a kpĩi tẽe na wʋ tɩ mʋɔl kʋ a kpĩisɩ bala na be a pɔɔfʋ die pɔ.
60003020	A banyãna lɛ tɔr a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ di kãnyir ka a Nowa wa maal a daka bulomtum baar. A nɩbɛ bɩ̃lãa na ɩ aniin tɛɛ wa nyɛn faafʋ a kʋ̃ɔ pɔ.
60003021	A kʋ̃ɔ nyã nyɛtãan fɩka a Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ sofʋ na faa yɩ mɩ a pʋ̃pãanyã, a ba ɩ ɩ̃gãn dɛɛr pɛɛ barfʋ lɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a nɛɛ yɩn tɩr kʋ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ pʋtɩvɩla. Yɩ nyɛn faafʋ tu a Kɩrɩsɩto kũu irfʋ pɔ.
60003022	'Lɔ lɛ do a saaju tɩ jɩ̃nɛ, a Nãaŋmɩn nũsʋ̃ɔ jie ka a malakasɩ, nɩ a tʋ̃ɔfʋ dẽme, nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme ba jaa turo a wʋ nɛɛ.
60004001	A lɛ jũu, a Kɩrɩsɩto na di dɔɔyɛ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn pɔ, yɩ mɩ su a tãjɛbonsɩ ala gun a tɩɛr 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, bojũu a 'lɔ na di dɔɔyɛ a wʋ ɩ̃gãn pɔ ba lɛ pʋɔ yelbier pɔ ɛ.
60004002	Ala lɛ so, wʋ ta lɛ kpɩɛrɛ a wɛr pɔ nɩ a ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ kpɩɛrɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔrɔ.
60004003	Bojũu a kõro jaa, yɩ mɩ sɔ̃ɔn sɔ̃ɔ na yɩ maala a lɛ a bala na ba puoro ɛ, na maala, na baa tʋɔrɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔrɔ ɛ. Ka a ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa, nɩ dãburo, nɩ a pepe dib, na yɩ pʋɔ a dãnyurbo gbul pɔ, na yɩ maala tɩbɛ na sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ.
60004004	Ban tɩɛr naa ɩka yelsãan lɛ, yɩn ba lɛ pʋɔ ba a befʋ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ pɔ ɛ, ka ba pãa piel tʋrɔ yɩ.
60004005	Tɩchɛ ban man a ba nɛɛ 'yɛr kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn na wa tɔɔr a vʋɛ nɩ a kpĩisɩ 'yɛr.
60004006	A anyãna jũu lɛ so ka ba gba mɩ mʋɔl a 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ kʋ a kpĩisɩ, ɩka ban tɔɔr a ba 'yɛr nɩtãa lɛ ban na tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr, tɩchɛ ka ba kpɩɛrɛ a sɩɩr pɔ Nãaŋmɩn kaar.
60004007	A bonsɩ a jaa baarfʋ tara naa, a lɛ jũu yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir na yɩ kpãa a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ tʋ̃ɔ sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn.
60004008	A ala na gar a jaa lɛ a anyã, yɩ chɛnɛ vɛ̃ ka a nʋ̃fʋ be a yɩ pɔ, bojũu nʋ̃fʋ ma pɔɔn yeldɛbɛ yɔɔ.
60004009	Yɩ ma diere taa a yɩ yie tɩ ta ma ɩrɛ gbʋrɔ̃ gbʋrɔ̃ ɛ.
60004010	Ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ de a Nãaŋmɩn kʋfʋ wʋn nyɛ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ nɩ a wʋ taaba nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ a jaa.
60004011	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛrɛ na, wʋ 'yɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbie ala. Ala ɩ wʋ ɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nɔ̃, wʋ tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ wʋ, ka a yele a jaa pɔ, ka Nãaŋmɩn nyɛ tɩɩr tu a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto pɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ so a tɩɩr nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ bɩbir bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
60004012	N yɛɛr nʋ̃nʋ̃nbɔ, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka nɛɛ 'maa yɩ nɩ a bɛɛr kaa tuo na vulo yɩ fɩka yelsãan kɔ̃ɔ lɛ ɩrɛ yɩ ɛ.
60004013	Tɩchɛ yɩ chɩlɛ an ɩ yɩ pʋɔ naa a Kɩrɩsɩto dɔɔyɛ difʋ pɔ, ka nʋ̃ɔ na kpɛ yɩ a wʋ tɩɩr wa nyɩr.
60004014	Ala ɩ ba tʋ yɩ naa yɩn bʋɔlɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto yuor jũu, Nãaŋmɩn na sʋ̃ʋ yɩ naa, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ben a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
60004015	Ala ɩ yɩ din dɔɔyɛ, a ta ɩ fɩka nɩkʋrɔ, bɩɩ nãnyie, bɩɩ nɩdɛɛr, bɩɩ tɔ'yɔ̃ɔnbɔ lɛ yɩ ɩ ɛ.
60004016	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa dire na dɔɔyɛ wʋn turo Kɩrɩsɩto jũu, wʋ ta vɛ̃ ka vɩ̃ kpɛ wʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ pɛɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn a yuor nyã wʋn di jũu.
60004017	Bojũu a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ sɔ̃ɔ ta naa, ka Nãaŋmɩn na piel tɔɔrɔ a wʋ nɩbɛ 'yɛr. Ala ɩ sɩn lɛ wʋn piel, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an kaara kʋ a bala na tɔr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nʋ̃ɔ?
60004018	A sɛb ɩka, "Ala ɩ an ɩn kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ a nɩtor, ŋmɩnɛ lɛ an kaara kʋ a bala na ba puor ɛ, nɩ a yelbe-ɩrbɛ?"
60004019	A lɛ jũu, vɛ̃ a bala na dire a dɔɔyɛ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ jũu, de ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ na mɛ ba, tɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir maala vɩla.
60005001	A maa na ɩ a nɩdiere naa nyɛ a Kɩrɩsɩto dɔɔyɛ nɩ nɩbir, naa mɩ ɩ nɩrɛ nyã na pʋɔ a tɩɩr 'lɔ na wa nyɩr, n 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ na a nɩdierbe na be be a yɩ pɔ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn,
60005002	ɩka ba kaara a Nãaŋmɩn piir a wʋn de 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩ nuur pɔ, na yɩ tʋ̃nɔ̃ kaara nɩ ba, a ta ɩ fɩrfʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a ɩ yɩ bɔfʋ, bojũu lɛ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn bʋɔrɔ. A ta ɩ libie 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ ka a nʋ̃mɔ̃ yɩ a tʋ̃fʋ.
60005003	Yɩ ta pirpire a bala yɩn kaar ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ɩ jɩ̃nɛ kʋ a piir.
60005004	A pɛchiin gbɔɔraa wa wa, yɩn nyɛn a sãyar na ɩ a tɩɩr na ba jʋɔl ɛ.
60005005	Lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ a yɩn bala na ɩ a pɔlbil, yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a yɩ nɩdierbe. Yɩ jaa jaa yɩ ma siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ na yɩ ma tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ taa, bojũu a sɛb ɩka, "Nãaŋmɩn 'laar a bala na 'mɔɔrɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ, tɩ ma sʋ̃nɔ̃ a bala na ma siir ba mɩ̃ɛ."
60005006	A lɛ jũu, yɩ siir yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn kpɛ̃ɔ sʋɔ nuur pɔ, ka wʋ 'mɔɔ yɩ a yɩ do a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ wʋn bʋɔrɔ.
60005007	Yɩ de a yɩ yelwõnsɩ a jaa kʋ wʋ, bojũu 'lɔ lɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a yɩ tɔɔ.
60005008	Yɩ gu yɩ mɩ̃ɛ na yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ jũmɔ̃, a yɩ dɔ̃sʋɔ tɩɩ kaara naa jukpɛ̃ɛ kaar, na uoro yʋɔrɔ na wʋ pãa kaara bʋɔrɔ nɩrɛ ɩka wʋ nyɔɔ 'wɔb.
60005009	Yɩ var wʋ sɔr, na yɩ ba gbɛr ara a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ, bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a yɩ taaba na be a wɛr wʋ jaa, mɩ dire na a dɔɔyɛ nyãna tɔ yɩn dire.
60005010	Yɩn wa di a dɔɔyɛ nyãna bɩ̃lãa a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a wɩ̃ɛfʋ sʋɔ a 'lɔ na bʋɔl yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a tɩɩr nyã na ba tara baarfʋ pɔ a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ, wʋ mɩ̃ɛ na maal yɩ naa na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ ɩ̃kpɛ̃ɔ tɩ na wʋ vɛ̃ a yɩ ara kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ̃ dãm ɛ.
60005011	'Lɔ lɛ so a kpɛ̃ɔ bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
60005012	Silasɩ na ɩ a yɛbɛ yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ lɛ sʋ̃ʋ ma ka n sɛb a gãn bile nyãna, naa 'yɔ̃ɔn yɩ ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn din dãasɩɛ ɩka anyãna lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn sɩrɛ wɩ̃ɛfʋ. Yɩ ara kpɛ̃ɔ.
60005013	A yɩ taaba pupuorbiir na be a Babilon Nãaŋmɩn na 'mataa ir yɩ, puor yɩ naa, ka a n bidaba Maakɩ mɩ puoro yɩ.
60005014	Yɩ puor puor taa nɩ nʋ̃fʋ. Nyã'maar wʋ be a yɩn bala na be a Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
61001001	Maa Simon Pita na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto gbãgbaa nɩ a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nãa lɛ sɛɛrɛ a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a yɩn na tu a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn yeltorsɩ pɔ, nɩ a sɩ Fafaara Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na yɩ nyɛ a sɔɔfʋ 'lɔ na kpɛ̃mɛ a sɩ kaar.
61001002	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar a dɔɔlɔ yɩ taa tu a bɔ̃ɔfʋ yɩn bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu.
61001003	A Wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ lɛ wʋ kʋn sɩ bon jaa sɩn bʋɔrɔ a nyɛvʋr nyã jũu nɩ Nãaŋmɩn puor vɩla tu a sɩ bɔ̃ɔfʋ sɩn bɔ̃ɔ a 'lɔ na bʋɔl sɩ, nɩ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ tɩɩr nɩ a wʋ maal vɩla.
61001004	Tu anyãna pɔ lɛ wʋ kʋn sɩ a bon na bɛrma nɩ a bʋ̃sʋ̃n wʋn tɩr a nɛɛ ɩka, a tu a pɔ, ka yɩn pʋɔ a befʋ 'lɔ na ba sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ɛ, na yɩ jo yi a wɛr nyã a yelbier vɔlaa na sɔ̃ɔ.
61001005	A anyãna jũu, yɩ mɔ̃ na yɩ de vɩla maalfʋ pʋɔ a yɩ sɔɔfʋ pɔ, na yɩ de bɔ̃ɔfʋ mɩ pʋɔ a vɩla maalfʋ pɔ,
61001006	ka a mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔfʋ mɩ pʋɔ a vɩla maalfʋ pɔ, ka a nɩbir mʋɔfʋ pʋɔ a mɩ̃ɛ nyɔɔfʋ pɔ, ka a Nãaŋmɩn puor vɩla pʋɔ a nɩbir mʋɔfʋ pɔ,
61001007	ka a yɛɛr maal vɩla pʋɔ a Nãaŋmɩn puor vɩla pɔ, na yɩ de nʋ̃fʋ pʋɔ a yɛɛr maal vɩla pɔ.
61001008	Bojũu ala ɩ yɩ tara naa anyãna a jaa ka a pʋɔrɔ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃, an sʋ̃ʋ yɩ naa ka yɩ kʋ̃ tara yãan na yaa tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃mɔ̃ a bɔ̃ɔfʋ yɩn bɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ɛ.
61001009	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ nɩrɛ baa tara a anyãna ɛ, waa nyɛrɛ ɛ, na wʋ ɩ jɔ̃ɔ, na wʋ ĩin ɩka Nãaŋmɩn pɛɛn a wʋ kõro jaa yeldɛbɛ bar.
61001010	A lɛ jũu n yɛɛr, yɩ ba gbɛr ka a yɩ bʋɔlfʋ nɩ a yɩ chɛl irfʋ ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ. Ala ɩ yɩn maala a anyãna, yaa be jaa na wa lo ɛ.
61001011	Ka a sɔr yuo kʋ yɩ a yɩ kpɛ a sɩ Soro nɩ a Fafaara Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nãalʋ̃ʋ na ba tara baarfʋ pɔ.
61001012	A lɛ ɩn ma jɛɔ yɩ naa a yelsɩ anyãna, yɩ gba na bɔ̃ɔ yaa ka yɩ ba gbɛr ara a yelmɩ̃ɛ yɩn tara pɔ.
61001013	A tara na sɔr ka n jɛɔ a yɩ tɩɛr ɩn chɛnɛ vʋrɔ a ɩ̃gãn vaar pɔ,
61001014	bojũu n bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a kʋ̃ lɛ kor ɛ tɩchɛ ka n kpi ɛ, nɩtãa lɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na man kʋ ma.
61001015	Ɩn ɩ naa lɛ jaa ɩn na tʋ̃ɔ, maa wa sɔɔ kpi, tɩ ka yɩ ma chɛnɛ tʋ̃ɔ tɩɛrɛ a yelsɩ anyãna.
61001016	A ba ɩ fuol nɩ yɛ̃ 'yɛr lɛ sɩ de 'yɛr kʋ yɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto waa ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩn mɩ̃ɛ lɛ nyɛ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɛ nɩ nɩbir.
61001017	Wʋ nyɛn 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ tɩɩr yi a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ lɛ a kɔkɔr na yi a tɩɩr jikpɛ̃ɛ jie wa a wʋ sɛ̃ 'yɛrɛ, "Nyã lɛ ɩ a n Bie 'lɔ ɩn nʋ̃, a wʋ yele pɛl naa n pʋɔ."
61001018	Sɩn mɩ̃ɛ wõn a kɔkɔr nyãna na yi a saaju wa, an ɩ sɩn nɩ 'lɔ jaa lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be a tɔ̃chɛchɛ par.
61001019	Sɩn lɛ tara a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ na dɔ̃ɔ be be 'yɛr na chaar, yɩ yuo toor chɛlɛ a 'yɛr. A kaara naa fɩka chãa na chaara libe pɔ, tɩ tãn a wɛr na chaar ka a bivɩɛ ŋmɛrbir pur 'yɔ̃ɔ a yɩ nyãn pɔ.
61001020	A yelkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ ɩka, yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a par ɩka Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ de a wʋ yɛ̃ wiil a ala na sɛb a Nãaŋmɩn gãn pɔ par ɛ.
61001021	Bojũu nɩrɛ maa kpu 'yɛr a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ ma 'yɛr a lɛ na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, an ɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ lɛ tara ba.
61002001	Tɩchɛ a jir ŋmarba 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ be be a nɩbɛ pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a jir ŋmarba wiwiilbe na wa be a yɩ pɔ. Ban sɔɔl wiil sɔ̃ɔfʋ 'yɛr, na ba chɩɩr a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ na da ba na ba waan sɔ̃ɔfʋ wa 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba mɩ̃ɛ.
61002002	Nɩyɔɔ na turo naa a ba vɩ̃ sɔɩ anyãna, tɩ na ba kpɛrɛ a yelmɩ̃ɛ sɔr.
61002003	A bɔgar wiwiilbe banyãna na 'mʋ̃ɔn yɩ naa nɩ a ba nɛnʋ̃ɔ 'yɛrbie. Nãaŋmɩn guor naa a ba 'yɛr kõro jaa ka a ba sɔ̃sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ ba guro ɛ.
61002004	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn ba dɔ̃ɔ bar a malakasɩ bala na maal a dɛɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ban a bɔɔ fulom libe 'lɔ pɔ bar chɛlɛ nɩ a ba 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar.
61002005	Waa dɔ̃ɔ bar a kõr nɩbɛ ɛ, na wʋ vɛ̃ ka a kʋ̃ɔ wa paal pɔɔ a bala na ba puoro ɛ, tɩ na wʋ faa a Nowa na ɩ yeltorsɩ 'yɛr mʋɔlɔ nɩ nɩbɛ ayopõi.
61002006	Nãaŋmɩn den bũu chʋm a Sodom nɩ a Gomora nɩbɛ ka a di lɩɛb tãpɩɛl, a nɩtɔ̃ wiil ɩka lɛ lɛ na ɩ a bala na ba puoro ɛ.
61002007	Wʋ mɩ faa naa Lotɩ na ɩ a nɩtor a wʋ pʋɔ na ma sɔ̃ɔn a bala na tʋ̃nɔ̃ a dɛbɛ.
61002008	Bojũu a nɩtor nyãna lɔ̃ɔn kpɩɛrɛ nɩ ba bɩbir jaa, ka a wʋ tɩɛr ma sɔ̃ɔ lɛ wʋn ma nyɛ tɩ wõ ban ɩrɛ.
61002009	An ɩ nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a be, a sɩ Soro bɔ̃ɔn lɛ wʋn pãa na ɩ faa a bala na puoro yin a wõm pɔ, tɩ tara a bala na ba puoro ɛ, a ba be a ba gefʋ pɔ tɩ tãn a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ bɩbir.
61002010	A anyãna ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ a bala na turo a ba ɩ̃gãn sɔ̃ɔnaa nyã dɛɛr vɔlaa, baa turo a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme nɛɛ ɛ. Ba ɩn jukpɩ̃ɛn dẽme na ba 'mɔɔrɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ, baa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩ ma kpɛrɛ a saaju bʋ̃maalsɩ.
61002011	Tɩchɛ a malakasɩ gba na ɩ gãdaar na ba tara kpɩ̃ɛn, ba maa 'la kpɛ a bʋ̃maalsɩ anyãna a sɩ Soro niem ɛ.
61002012	Tɩchɛ a nɩbɛ banyãna ma fere naa nɩ a bonsɩ ala ban ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ. Ba kaara naa mɔdʋ̃n kaar bʋ̃maalaa na ba tara tɩɛrɛ, ba dɔɔ ba naa na nyɔɔr ba kʋ, ba mɩ kaara a mɔdʋ̃n kaar na ba mɩ na wɛ.
61002013	A dɛɛr ala ban maal, a dɛɛr ala lɛ ban yãan ba a sãn. A ba tɩɛr vɔlaa ban ma maala a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ, a nʋ̃mɔ̃ ba naa, ban lɔ̃ɔn dire nɩ yɩ na ban sɔ̃ɔ a yɩ befʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ yɩ vɩ̃.
61002014	A ba nɩbie sɛɛn naa a sɛ̃sɛ̃yele, a ba maa bar dɛɛr ɩfʋ ɛ. Ba ma bɛlɛ naa a bala na bal na ba ɩ bɔgar dẽme, ba ben pɔ'yɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ.
61002015	Ba bar a sɔr dẽ dẽ 'lɔ tɩ bɔr, na ba tu a Balaam na ɩ a Beor bidaba sɔr. 'Lɔ lɛ nʋ̃ sãyar na ba ɩ ɛ,
61002016	tɩchɛ wʋ nyɛn a wʋ bawõno tɔ̃nɔ̃, bʋ̃ɔ na ɩ dʋ̃ɔ den nɩrɛ kɔkɔr 'yɛr 'yɛr na wʋ ŋmaan a 'yɛ'yɛrɛ nyãna dãbol yele sɔr.
61002017	A nɩbɛ banyãna ɩ naa fɩka kʋlsɩ na ba tara kʋ̃ɔ ɛ, bɩɩ uul sɛsɛbɛ na furo chiine. Libe jaa gbɛb lɛ guro ba.
61002018	Bojũu yobɔ 'yɛr pɔrsɩ lɛ ba ma 'yɛrɛ, na ba bʋɔlɔ a ɩ̃gãn vɔldɛɛr, na ba bɛlɛ nɩ a nɩbɛ bala na faa joro a bala na bɔr sɛ̃.
61002019	Ba ma tɩr nɛɛ kʋ ba ɩka ban faa ban a gbãgbayele pɔ, tɩchɛ ka a bala mɩ̃ɛ ɩ a yelsɔ̃ɔnsɩ gbãgbaar, bojũu nɩrɛ ɩn gbãgbaa kʋ bon 'lɔ jaa na tʋ̃ɔ wʋ.
61002020	Ala ɩ ba faan ba mɩ̃ɛ yin a wɛr nyã bɔdɛɛr pɔ, ban wa bɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Soro nɩ a Fafaara Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tɩ na ba lɛ tɩ kpɛ a ala pɔ ka a tʋ̃ɔ ba, a ba baarfʋ na ɩn dɛɛr gar a lɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ be.
61002021	An taa sa naa ala ɩ baa ta bɔ̃ɔ a sɔr toraa ɛ, gar ban ben bɔ̃ɔn tɩ lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɛbin chɛchɛ 'lɔ ban de kʋ ba.
61002022	Bala 'lɔ, a sʋkpa nyã ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ lɔb ɩka, baa lɩɛb tɩ di a ala wʋn ti bar, ka a dobaa ban so kʋ̃ɔ mɩ lɩɛb tɩ mamar a mɛmɛrɛ.
61003001	N barmɩne, a gãma ayi sʋɔ lɛ anyã ɩn sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ. A jaa ayi pɔ, n sɛb ɩka n lɛ jɛɔ yɩ tɩɛr 'lɔ na tor pɔ.
61003002	N bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka yɩ lɩɛb tɩɛr a 'yɛrbie ala a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrchɛchɛ bala na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a sɩ Soro nɩ a Fafaara na dɔ̃ɔ man ba tu a wʋ nɩtʋ̃nsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
61003003	Yɩ de nie bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a ber baaraa sɔ̃ɔ, nɩlaarba na turo a ba ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa na wa naa wa laara yɩ.
61003004	Ban wa sʋrɔ yɩ naa, "Nyɩnɛ lɛ a 'lɔ na tɩr a nɛɛ kʋ yɩ ɩka wʋn wa naa? A lɛ daar jaa a sɩ sãamɩne na kpi a yelsɩ a jaa mɩ chɛnɛ na chiine a lɛ nɛ an piel."
61003005	Tɩchɛ ba bɔ̃ɔn naa tɩ maala fɩka ba ĩin naa a kõro jaa an ɩ Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrbie lɛ wʋ maal a saaju, nɩ a tẽe a kʋ̃ɔ ju, nɩ a kʋ̃ɔ par.
61003006	A tẽkor, kʋ̃ɔ mɩ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ paal pɔɔ a wɛr a wʋ sɔ̃ɔ.
61003007	A 'yɛr nyãna nɩ wʋ ju lɛ wʋ bar a saaju, nɩ a tẽe go gun a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ, na wʋn sɔ̃ɔn a bala na ba puoro ɛ, nɩ bũu.
61003008	Tɩchɛ yɩ ta ĩin a yelbʋ̃'yen nyãna ɛ, n barmɩne. A sɩ Soro sɛ̃, bɩbir bʋ̃'yen kaara naa fɩka yuon tur, ka a yuon tur kaara fɩka bɩbir bʋ̃'yen a wʋ sɛ̃.
61003009	A sɩ Soro ba baala nɩ a wʋ nɛɛ wʋn tɩr ɛ, nɩtãa lɛ a bamɩne na 'yɛr ɩka a kor naa ɛ. Wʋ din kãnyir kʋ yɩ, wʋn ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wʋ wɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ lɩɛb a yɩ tɩɛr.
61003010	A sɩ Soro bɩbir na wa naa fɩka lɛ nãnyie na ma wa, ka a saaju pɔɔn gɔ̃mɔ̃ wʋ jaa, na wʋ po chen. A bonsɩ ala na be a saaju ka a bũu nyɩl na wʋ pãa yuo yele a jaa a nɩbɛ na maala ka a gã chãa pɔ.
61003011	An ɩ a bonsɩ a jaa na wa sɔ̃ɔn a nɩtɔ̃nɔ̃, nɩbotɔ lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka yɩ ɩ? A sɛɛ naa ka a yɩ maalfʋ ɩ chɛchɛ, na yɩ puoro Nãaŋmɩn,
61003012	nɩtãa lɛ yɩn ben kaara a Nãaŋmɩn waa bɩbir na yɩ 'mi'mine nɩ a wʋ waa. A bɩbir nyãna na waan nɩ sɔ̃ɔfʋ, a saaju wʋ jaa na di naa, ka a bonsɩ a jaa mɩ nyɩl nɩ a tʋl.
61003013	Tɩchɛ sɩn chɛlɛ naa tẽpaalaa nɩ a saaju paalaa na ɩ a nɩtorsɩ tẽe, 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na tɩr a nɛɛ.
61003014	A lɛ n barmɩne, yɩn pãa na chɛlɛ a anyãna jũu, yɩ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir na yɩ taa tara chɛfʋ nɩ mabfʋ jie ɛ, na yɩ tara wʋ nɩ nyã'maar.
61003015	Yɩ tɩɛr a anyã ɩka a sɩ Soro kãnyir ɩ naa a yɩ faafʋ lɛ, nɩtãa lɛ a sɩ yɛbɛ Pɔɔl mɩ na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb kʋ yɩ nɩ a yɛ̃ 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ wʋ.
61003016	A wʋ gãma a jaa pɔ, a 'yɛr bʋ̃'yen lɛ wʋ sɛb, na wʋ 'yɛrɛ a yelsɩ anyãna. A wʋ gãma pɔ yelsɩ ben be na ɩ tuo a par bɔ̃ɔfʋ, ka a ba bɔ̃ɔ nɩ a a bala na ba bɔ̃ɔ ara dẽme lɩɛb a bur bur nɩtãa lɛ ban lɩɛr a Nãaŋmɩn gãma amɩne, ka a na ɩ ba mɩ̃ɛ sɔ̃ɔfʋ.
61003017	A lɛ jũu, n barmɩne, yɩn ben de nie bɔ̃ɔn a nɩtɔ̃, yɩ guro a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ka a ba bɛlfʋ ta wa vɛ̃ ka yɩ faa lo tɩ bar a yɩ gbɛr bafʋ jie ɛ.
61003018	Tɩchɛ yɩ nʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ a sɩ Soro nɩ a Fafaara Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ a wʋ bɔ̃ɔfʋ pɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ so a tɩɩr a pʋ̃pãanyã, nɩ bɩbir, nɩ a bɩbir jaa. A ɩ a lɛ.
62001001	Maa Jɔɔn sɛɛrɛ na kʋrɔ a yɩn na turo a Yesu. A 'yɛr na dɔ̃ɔ be be a wɛr pielfʋ daar, 'lɔ lɛ sɩ wõ a wʋ yele na sɩ nyɛ wʋ. Sɩ nyɛ wʋ naa nɩ a sɩ nɩbie na sɩ sɩɩr wʋ nɩ a sɩ mɩ̃ɛ nuur. A 'yɛr nyã lɛ ɩ a nyɛvʋr.
62001002	A nyɛvʋr nyã lɛ yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ka wʋ de wiil sɩ a sɩ nyɛ wʋ, 'lɔ lɛ sɩ dire a wʋ dãasɩɛ na sɩ mʋɔlɔ kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. 'Lɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, ka wʋ wa ir wʋ wiil sɩ.
62001003	Sɩ 'yɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ a lɛ a sɩn mɩ̃ɛ na nyɛ tɩ wõ, ka a lɛ na vɛ̃ ka sɩn nɩ yɩn na tara nɛbʋ̃'yen, ka a sɩn nɩ a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn 'matãan a wʋ Bie Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tara a nɛbʋ̃'yen.
62001004	A nyã lɛ sɩ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ kaa sɩ chɩlfʋ na sɛɛ.
62001005	A 'yɛr wʋn kʋ sɩ ka sɩ mʋɔlɔ kʋrɔ yɩ nɩ nyã, Nãaŋmɩn ɩn chãa ka libe ba be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ jaa ɛ.
62001006	Ala ɩ sɩ 'yɛr naa ɩka sɩn nɩ 'lɔ tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen tɩ chɛnɛ chiine a libe pɔ, sɩ ɩn jir ŋmarba na saa turo a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
62001007	Tɩchɛ ala ɩ sɩ chiine naa a chãa pɔ nɩtãa lɛ a 'lɔ na be a chãa pɔ, sɩn tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen ka a wʋ Bie Yesu jɩ̃ɩ pɛɛ a sɩ yeldɛbɛ a jaa bar.
62001008	Ala ɩ sɩ 'yɛr ɩka saa tara yeldɛɛr jaa ɛ, sɩ bɛlɛ na sɩ mɩ̃ɛ, na saa tara yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
62001009	Ala ɩ sɩ 'yɛr naa a sɩ yeldɛbɛ kʋ Nãaŋmɩn, wʋn vɛ̃n kʋ sɩ, tɩ pɛɛ a sɩ yeldɛbɛ a jaa bar, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ nɩ nɩtor.
62001010	Ala ɩ sɩ 'yɛr naa ɩka saa maal yeldɛɛr jaa ɛ, sɩ bʋɔlɔ na Nãaŋmɩn jir ŋmara, na saa de a wʋ 'yɛr a sɩ nyãa pɔ ɛ.
62002001	N bibiir, n sɛɛrɛ naa anyã kʋrɔ yɩ ka yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa taa wa ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ wa ɩn yeldɛɛr, sɩ tara na po pire na be a Sãa sɛ̃. 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na ɩ a Torfʋ Sʋɔ.
62002002	'Lɔ lɛ lo a sɩ yeldɛbɛ bɔɔr kʋ sɩ, a ba ɩ sɩn tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ a wɛr wʋ jaa.
62002003	A nɩtɔ̃ lɛ sɩ de bɔ̃ɔn ɩka sɩ be naa a wʋ sɛ̃, sɩn turo a wʋ nɛbinsɩ jũu.
62002004	Nɩrɛ 'yɛr ɩka wʋ bɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn tɩ ba ɩrɛ a lɛ wʋn bin a nɛɛ ɛ, a nɩnyɩnɛ ɩn jir ŋmara na waa tara yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
62002005	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ jaa na turo a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr, sɩrɛ jaa Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃fʋ sɛɛn a wʋ pɔ. Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ sɩ de bɔ̃ɔn ɩka sɩ be naa a wʋ pɔ.
62002006	Nɩrɛ jaa na 'yɛr ɩka wʋ be naa Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ, wʋ chiine a lɛ a Yesu na dɔ̃ɔ chen.
62002007	N barmɩne, a ba ɩ nɛbin paalaa lɛ n sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bʋ̃koraa 'lɔ yɩn tara yi a pielfʋ lɛ, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a nɛkoraa yɩn wõ.
62002008	Tɩchɛ wʋ ɩn bʋ̃paalaa, bojũu a ɩn sɩrɛ a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ, naa mɩ ɩ sɩrɛ a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, bojũu a libe tɔɔn 'laa, ka a sɩrɛ chãa chaara.
62002009	Nɩrɛ jaa wa 'yɛr ɩka maa ben chãa pɔ, tɩ 'laar a wʋ yɛbɛ, wʋ chɛnɛ na be a libe pɔ.
62002010	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na nʋ̃ a wʋ yɛbɛ ben a chãa pɔ, ka bon jaa ba be be na vɛ̃ ka wʋ ŋme gbɛr ɛ.
62002011	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na 'laar a wʋ yɛbɛ ben a libe pɔ, na wʋ yʋɔrɔ a libe pɔ, na waa bɔ̃ɔ a jie wʋn chiine ɛ, bojũu a libe jɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa.
62002012	N bibiir, n sɛɛrɛ na a gãn nyã kʋrɔ yɩ bojũu Nãaŋmɩn vɛ̃ naa a yɩ yeldɛbɛ kʋ yɩ a lɛ a Yesu na ɩ kʋ yɩ jũu.
62002013	Sãamɩne, n sɛɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ bojũu, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a 'lɔ na yi a wɛr pielfʋ. Pɔlbil, n sɛɛrɛ na kʋrɔ yɩ bojũu yɩ tʋ̃ɔn a dɛɛr sʋɔ. Naa mɩ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ a yɩn bibiir bojũu yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn.
62002014	N sɛb kʋ a yɩn sãamɩne bojũu, yɩ bɔ̃ɔn a 'lɔ na yi a wɛr pielfʋ daar. N sɛb kʋ a yɩn pɔlbil a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr na be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ jũu, yɩ kpɛ̃mɛ na, na yɩ jɛb tʋ̃ɔ a dɛɛr sʋɔ.
62002015	Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa nʋ̃nɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃sɩ bɩɩ bon jaa ban tara ɛ. Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa nʋ̃n a lɛ, a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃fʋ ba be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
62002016	Bojũu a bonsɩ anyã sɩn nyɛ ɩ naa a ɩ̃gãn nyã vɔlaa nɩ a nɩbie vɔlaa bɩɩ tara jɩ̃ jɩɩr nɩ bʋ̃tarsɩ. A nyãna a jaa wʋn na ɩrɛ ba yi a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ, tɩchɛ a yi naa dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃sɩ sɛ̃.
62002017	A bɔdɛbɛ anyã mɩ poro na chiine, tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ɩrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn bɔfʋ na ben be sɔ̃ɔ jaa.
62002018	N bibiir, a wɛr baarfʋ ta naa, nɩtãa lɛ yɩn dɔ̃ɔ wõ ɩka a bala na 'laar a Kɩrɩsɩto na wa naa, ba yɔɔ lɛ a banyãna na be ka gba. Ala lɛ sɩ de bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a baraa sɔ̃ɔ lɛ.
62002019	A nɩbɛ banyãna dɔ̃ɔ be a sɩ sɛ̃ tɩ wa yi. Ka a ba yifʋ wiil ɩka baa tara sɩ nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen ɛ, sɩn nɩ bala ta ɩ bʋ̃'yen, ban taa be naa sɩ sɛ̃, tɩchɛ a ba yifʋ wiil ɩka baa pʋɔ sɩ ɛ.
62002020	Tɩchɛ yɩn 'lɔ, Yesu kʋ yɩ naa a wʋ Sɩɛ ka yɩ jaa bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ.
62002021	N ba sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ yɩ bojũu yɩn ba bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩn bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ lɛ. Bojũu yɩ mɩ bɔ̃ɔn a jir na tɛɛ nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
62002022	An lɛ ɩ a jir ŋmara? Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'yɛr ɩka a Yesu ba ɩ a Nɩ-iraa ɛ, a nɩrɛ 'lɔ lɛ 'laar a Kɩrɩsɩto. A nɩnyɩnɛ tɔr naa a Sãa nɩ a Bie jaa.
62002023	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tɔr a Bie mɩ tɔr a Sãa, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na 'yɛr chãa pɔ ɩka Yesu lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩ a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn.
62002024	Yɩ chɛnɛ tara a lɛ nɛ yɩn wõ a Yesu 'yɛr a pielfʋ, yɩn wa chɛnɛ tara a lɛ, yɩn tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩ a Sãa nɩ a wʋ Bie.
62002025	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr ɩka wʋn ɩ naa wʋn vɛ̃ naa ka sɩ tara nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
62002026	N sɛɛrɛ na a anyãna kʋrɔ yɩ ɩka yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃ nɩ a bala na bar yɩ tɩ yi, ba bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba bɛl yɩ yin.
62002027	A yɩn 'lɔ, ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bɛl yɩ ɛ, bojũu Yesu kʋ yɩ naa a Sɩɛ ka wʋ be a yɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ. A Sɩɛ na ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ na wile yɩ jũu, yaa lɛ bʋɔrɔ ɩka nɩrɛ wʋ wiil yɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ go ɛ, tɩchɛ a Sɩɛ a Yesu na kʋ yɩ vɛ̃ naa ka yɩ bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ, ka ala mɩ a Sɩɛ na wile ɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, jir jaa ba be be ɛ. A lɛ jũu, yɩ chɛnɛ tara a Yesu nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩtãa lɛ a Sɩɛ na 'yɛr yɩ.
62002028	A lɛ jũu n bibiir, yɩ chɛnɛ tara a Yesu nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen, ka 'lɔ wa yi a saaju lɩɛb waara a wɛr pɔ, sɩn tara na nyãa ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kʋ̃ kʋrɔ sɩ a wʋ tuorfʋ ɛ.
62002029	Yɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka a Yesu yele tor naa, nɩrɛ jaa mɩ na maala a lɛ, mɩ ɩ naa a Nãaŋmɩn bie.
62003001	Nyɛ lɛ a sɩ Sãa na nʋ̃ sɩ jɩ̃. Wʋ sɔɔn bʋɔlɔ sɩ a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir, ka sɩ mɩ sɩr ɩ! A lɛ jũu, a wɛr nɩbɛ ba bɔ̃ɔ wʋ ɛ, ala lɛ so ban ba bɔ̃ɔ sɩ ɛ.
62003002	N barmɩne, pʋ̃pãanyã, sɩ ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn bibiir, saa bɔ̃ɔ lɛ sɩn na be daar kɔ̃ɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka, a Yesu wa lɩɛb wa a wɛr nyã pɔ, sɩn nyɛ naa a lɛ wʋn na be, na sɩ kaara a wʋ kaar.
62003003	Yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na tara a tɩɛrtɔ nyãna a Yesu 'yɔ̃ɔ, wʋ ir wʋ mɩ̃ɛ yin dɛɛr pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a Yesu na ɩ chɛchɛ.
62003004	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na chɛnɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr, a nɩnyɩnɛ sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ naa a Nãaŋmɩn nɛbinsɩ ala wʋn bin, bojũu waa tara Nãaŋmɩn nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen ɛ.
62003005	Tɩchɛ yɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Yesu ba maal dɛɛr ɛ, a lɛ ka wʋ wa ɩka wʋ wa de a sɩ dɛbɛ bar.
62003006	A lɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na tara Yesu nɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen, wʋ maa lɛ chɛnɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr go ɛ, tɩchɛ a nɩnyɩnɛ wa chɛnɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr, waa bɔ̃ɔ a Yesu nɩ a nɩnyɩnɛ wʋn ɩ ɛ.
62003007	N bibiir yɩ bɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sʋ̃, ka nɩrɛ jaa taa bɛlɛ yɩ ɛ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na maala a lɛ na tor, wʋ ɩ naa nɩtor nɩtãa lɛ Yesu na ɩ nɩtor.
62003008	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na chɛnɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr yi naa a tɩɩ sɛ̃, bojũu 'lɔ lɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛbɛ yi a wɛr pielfʋ. Ala lɛ so ka Yesu na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn Bie wa ɩka wʋ wa sɔ̃ɔ a tɩɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃.
62003009	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na wa ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bie, maa lɛ sɛɛ ɩka wʋ lɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛbɛ go ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn befʋ be naa a wʋ yɔ̃ɔ. Wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ chɛnɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛbɛ go ɛ, bojũu wʋ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn bie.
62003010	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ sɩ de bɔ̃ɔn a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir nɩ a Tɩɩ bibiir. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ba wa turo a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ 'lɔ wʋn bin bɩɩ na waa lɛ nʋ̃ a wʋ yɛɛr, waa ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bie ɛ.
62003011	An yi a daar 'lɔ jaa yɩn piel sɔɔ Yesu, yɩ wõ naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr bie na 'yɛr ɩka sɩ nʋ̃ taa.
62003012	Yɩ ta ɩ a sɩ kaara a Kain kaar ɛ, wʋ tara na a dɛɛr sʋɔ tɩɛr na wʋ kʋ a wʋ yɛbile. Bo lɛ so wʋn kʋ a yɛbile? Bojũu a Kain tʋ̃mɔ̃ ɩn dɛɛr, tɩchɛ ka a wʋ yɛbile tʋ̃mɔ̃ tor.
62003013	N yɛɛr, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka a fɛr yɩ ala ɩ a nɩbɛ na be a wɛr pɔ wa 'laar yɩ naa ɛ.
62003014	Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka sɩ nʋ̃ naa a sɩ taaba. A wiil ɩka sɩ yin kũu pɔ, tɩ kpɛ nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ pɔ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba nʋ̃ a wʋ yɛbɛ ɛ, wʋ chɛnɛ na be kũu pɔ.
62003015	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na 'laar a wʋ yɛɛr ɩn nɩkʋrɔ a wʋ nyãa pɔ, ka yɩ mɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka nɩkʋrɔ ba tara nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
62003016	Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn lɛ a nʋ̃fʋ na be, bojũu Yesu sɔɔn kpi kʋ sɩ, ka a mɩ sɛɛ ɩka, sɩ mɩ sɔɔ kpi kʋ a sɩ yɛɛr.
62003017	Ala ɩ a yɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ tara naa ka a sɛɛn wʋ, tɩ nyɛ a wʋ taa yɛɛr an wõnõ ka wʋ lɩɛb puor yɔ̃ɔ ba, a Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃fʋ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ be a wʋ sʋɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
62003018	N bibiir, yɩ ta vɛ̃ ka sɩ nʋ̃fʋ ɩ 'yɛrbie nɩ jãlbir 'yɛrbie ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ ɩ ka sɩ sʋ̃nɔ̃ taa nɩtãa lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na nʋ̃ sɩ sɩrɛ jaa.
62003019	A sɩ befʋ pɔ lɛ sɩn bɔ̃ɔ ɩka sɩ be naa a yelmɩ̃ɛ pɔ sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa sɩn wa ara a Nãaŋmɩn niem sʋɔrɔ wʋ, sɩ kʋ̃ lɛ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ,
62003020	ala gba ɩ a sɩ tɩɛr 'yɛr ɩka sɩ maal dɛɛr. Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn bɔ̃ɔn yele jaa a sɩ nyãn pɔ, na wʋ bɔ̃ɔ yele jaa sɩn ɩrɛ.
62003021	N barmɩne, ala ɩ sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa a sɩ tɩɛr pɔ, ɩka sɩ maa chɛnɛ maala dɛɛr ɛ, sɩn wa sʋɔrɔ Nãaŋmɩn, sɩ kʋ̃ joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ,
62003022	sɩn nyɛn bon jaa sɩn sʋɔr yi a wʋ sɛ̃, bojũu sɩ turo naa a wʋ nɛɛ na sɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ na pɛlɛ a wʋ pʋɔ.
62003023	Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ wʋn bin nɩ nyã, ɩka sɩ sɔɔ a wʋ Bie Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto yuor na sɩ nʋ̃ a sɩ taaba, nɩtãa a lɛ wʋn 'yɛr sɩ.
62003024	Bala jaa na turo a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ wʋn bin, ba ben a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka wʋ mɩ be a ba 'yɔ̃ɔ. Sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka wʋ ben a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, a Sɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn de kʋ sɩ jũu.
62004001	N barmɩne, yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa sɔɔ nɩrɛ jaa na 'yɛr ɩka wʋ tara na a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ yɩ bɛɛr a nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ kaa, ka ala ɩ a 'yɛr wʋn 'yɛrɛ yin a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃. Bojũu jir 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ yi naa jie jaa na ba 'yɛrɛ ɩka a lɛ ban 'yɛrɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ ba.
62004002	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ yɩn de bɔ̃ɔn a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, nɩrɛ 'lɔ nɩ wa 'yɛr ɩka Yesu wa naa a wɛr pɔ nɩtãa nɩsaal, a nɩrɛ 'lɔ lɛ yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
62004003	Nɩrɛ jaa wa tɔr a lɛ ba yi Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ, a nɩrɛ nyã lɛ 'laar a Kɩrɩsɩto, a 'lɔ yɩn wõ ɩka wʋn wa naa, 'lɔ lɛ be be a wɛr pɔ a pʋ̃pãanyã.
62004004	N bibiir, yɩn 'lɔ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ na yɩ tʋ̃ɔ ba, bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'lɔ na be a yɩ pɔ, bɛrma naa gar a dɛɛr sʋɔ 'lɔ na be a wɛr pɔ.
62004005	A jir dẽme banyãna na 'yɛr ɩka Nãaŋmɩn lɛ kʋ ba a wiilfʋ anyãna ɩ naa a wɛr nyã nɩbɛ. Ka a ba wiilfʋ ɩ a wɛr nyã pɔ wiilfʋ, ka a bala na ba ɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ɛ, ma sɔɔ a ba wiilfʋ.
62004006	Sɩn 'lɔ ɩn naa a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn, ma sɔɔ naa a lɛ sɩn wile, tɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, maa sɔɔ a lɛ sɩn wile ɛ. Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ sɩn tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔn ka a nɩnyɩnɛ na 'yɛrɛ tara naa Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'lɔ na ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ, bɩɩ nɩrɛ 'lɔ na yi a Satan sɛ̃ na ɩ a jir ŋmara.
62004007	N barmɩne, yɩ vɛ̃ a sɩ wile taa nʋ̃fʋ. N 'yɛr naa a nɩtɔ̃ bojũu Nãaŋmɩn lɛ ma vɛ̃ a sɩ ma tʋ̃ɔ nʋ̃ taa. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na wa nʋ̃ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ, a wiil ɩka Nãaŋmɩn bie lɛ wʋ ɩ na wʋ bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn.
62004008	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na baa wa nʋ̃ a wʋ taaba ɛ, ba bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn befʋ wʋ jaa ɩn nʋ̃fʋ.
62004009	A sɔr nyã lɛ Nãaŋmɩn tu wiil a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ kʋ sɩ. Wʋ vɛ̃n a wʋ Bibʋ̃'yen tɛɛ ka wʋ wa a wɛr pɔ, a wʋ jũu, sɩ tara na a yelmɩ̃ɛ nyɛvʋr.
62004010	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a nʋ̃fʋ be, a ba ɩ sɩn lɛ nʋ̃ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, tɩchɛ 'lɔ lɛ nʋ̃ sɩ, na wʋ tʋ̃ a wʋ Bie ka wʋ wa lo a sɩ yeldɛbɛ bɔɔr kʋ sɩ.
62004011	N barmɩne, an ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ nʋ̃ sɩ a nɩtɔ̃, a mɩ sɛɛ naa ɩka, sɩ mɩ nʋ̃ taa.
62004012	Nɩrɛ jaa ba nyɛ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ wʋn be ɛ, tɩchɛ sɩn wa nʋ̃ taa, sɩn nɩ Nãaŋmɩn tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen. Ka a Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃fʋ 'lɔ na be a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ chaar kʋ a nɩbɛ.
62004013	Nãaŋmɩn kʋ sɩ naa a wʋ Sɩɛ, a lɛ jũu lɛ sɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka, Nãaŋmɩn ben a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka sɩ mɩ be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ, ala lɛ so sɩn nɩ Nãaŋmɩn na tara nɛbʋ̃'yen.
62004014	Sɩ nyɛ naa na sɩ mɩ di dãasɩɛ ɩka a Sãa tʋ̃ naa a wʋ Bie ka wʋ wa faa a wɛr nɩbɛ.
62004015	Nãaŋmɩn tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩ nɩrɛ nyã na 'yɛr chãa pɔ, tɩ sɔɔ ɩka Yesu ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn Bie, ka sɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a nɩnyɩnɛ tara na nɛbʋ̃'yen.
62004016	A lɛ sɩn 'lɔ, sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa na sɩ sɔɔ de ɩka, Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃ sɩn sɔ̃ɔ jaa. Nãaŋmɩn ɩn nʋ̃fʋ sʋɔ. Nɩrɛ mɩ na nʋ̃ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a wʋ taaba, wʋ ben Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka Nãaŋmɩn mɩ be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ.
62004017	Sɩn 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃fʋ chaara a sɩ pɔ, ka dãbɩ̃ɛ kʋ̃ kʋrɔ sɩ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ sɩn wa ara a wʋ niem a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ daar ɛ. Bojũu a wɛr nyã pɔ sɩ kaar naa nɩtãa Yesu.
62004018	Dãbɩ̃ɛ ba be nʋ̃fʋ pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ nʋ̃fʋ na chaar ma diin dãbɩ̃ɛ bar, bojũu dãbɩ̃ɛ ma kpɛ̃n nɩrɛ wʋn joro gefʋ. Nʋ̃fʋ mɩ na chaar, ba joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ.
62004019	Bojũu Nãaŋmɩn lɛ de nie nʋ̃ sɩ, ala lɛ so a sɩ mɩ nʋ̃ wʋ.
62004020	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ 'yɛr ɩka wʋ nʋ̃n Nãaŋmɩn, tɩ chɛnɛ 'laar a wʋ yɛɛr, a nɩnyɩnɛ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩn jir ŋmara. Bojũu nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na ba nʋ̃ a wʋ tɔ sʋɔ wʋn nyɛn nɩbir, kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ nʋ̃ Nãaŋmɩn wʋn ba nyɛn nɩbir ɛ.
62004021	A nɛɛ lɛ a nyã a Nãaŋmɩn na 'yɛr bin, nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na nʋ̃ a 'lɔ Nãaŋmɩn sɛɛ naa ɩka wʋ nʋ̃ a wʋ taaba.
62005001	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ ɩka Yesu lɛ ɩ a Nɩ-iraa, ɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn bie. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na nʋ̃ a sãa mɩ nʋ̃ naa a bie.
62005002	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ sɩn de bɔ̃ɔn ɩka sɩ nʋ̃ naa a Nãaŋmɩn bibiir ala ɩ sɩ nʋ̃n a Nãaŋmɩn na sɩ turo a wʋ nɛɛ wʋn bin.
62005003	Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ sɩn de bɔ̃ɔn ɩka sɩ nʋ̃n Nãaŋmɩn sɩrɛ jaa, ala ɩ sɩ tun a lɛ jaa wʋn 'yɛr ka sɩ tu. A ba ɩ tuo ka sɩ na tu a lɛ jaa wʋn 'yɛr ɩka sɩ tu ɛ.
62005004	Bojũu nɩrɛ jaa na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bie ma lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɔr dɛbɛ ala a nɩbɛ na turo. A lɛ vɛ̃ naa, ka wʋ ma tʋ̃ɔ tɔr a sɔr dɛbɛ ala a nɩbɛ na turo, Yesu wʋn sɔɔ jũu.
62005005	An lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ lɩɛb puor 'yɔ̃ɔ a wɛr? Nɩrɛ 'lɔ tɛɛ na sɔɔ ɩka Yesu lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie.
62005006	A Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nyã lɛ wa a ba so wʋ Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ɔ nɩ a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ. Waa so a kʋ̃ɔ tɛɛ ɛ, tɩ wʋ kpi naa na wʋ kpaar a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ, ka a Sɩɛ mɩ di a wʋ dãasɩɛ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ma 'yɛrɛ naa yelmɩ̃ɛ.
62005007	Bojũu dãasɩɛsɩ ata lɛ be be,
62005008	a Sɩɛ, nɩ a kʋ̃ɔ, nɩ a jɩ̃ɩ, ka a jaa ata dãasɩɛ ɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen.
62005009	Ala ɩ sɩ ma sɔɔ naa nɩsaal dãasɩɛ, sɩn sɔɔ naa Nãaŋmɩn dãasɩɛ 'lɔ wʋn di a wʋ Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ, bojũu Nãaŋmɩn dãasɩɛ bɛrma naa gar nɩsaal dãasɩɛ.
62005010	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na sɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie, a dãasɩɛ nyã be naa a wʋ nyãa pɔ. Nɩrɛ nyã jaa na ba wa sɔɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, wʋ bʋɔl wʋn jir ŋmara bojũu waa sɔɔ a dãasɩɛ wʋn di a wʋ Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ ɛ.
62005011	A dãasɩɛ nɩ nyã, Nãaŋmɩn kʋ sɩ naa nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, ka a nyɛvʋr nyã be a wʋ Bie 'yɔ̃ɔ.
62005012	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara a Bie, tara na nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba wa tara a Bie ɛ, ba tara nyɛvʋr ɛ.
62005013	N sɛb kʋ a yɩn bala na sɔɔ a Nãaŋmɩn Bie yuor, ka yɩn bɔ̃ɔ ɩka yɩ tara na nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
62005014	A 'lafʋ nyã lɛ sɩ tara ɩka, sɩn wa sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn a lɛ wʋn bʋɔrɔ, wʋn wõ naa naa.
62005015	Ka ala ɩ sɩ bɔ̃ɔn na ɩka Nãaŋmɩn wõ naa a lɛ sɩn ma sʋɔr wʋ, sɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka sɩ tara na bon jaa sɩn sʋɔr wʋ.
62005016	Ala ɩ yɩ wa nyɛ naa a yɩ tɔ sʋɔ na ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr kɔ̃ɔ na kʋ̃ sʋ̃ʋ wʋ ɛ, yɩ sʋɔr Nãaŋmɩn ka wʋ vɛ̃ kʋ wʋ. Tɩchɛ yeldɛbɛ amɩne ben be fʋn na ɩ ka Nãaŋmɩn kʋ̃ vɛ̃ kʋ fʋ ɛ, n ba 'yɛr ɩka yɩ sʋɔr a ala ɛ.
62005017	Yeldɛbɛ a jaa ɩn yelbier, tɩchɛ yelbier a jaa baa kʋrɔ kũu ɛ.
62005018	Sɩn bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na wa ɩ Nãaŋmɩn bie, kʋ̃ lɛ chɛnɛ ɩrɛ yeldɛɛr ɛ, Nãaŋmɩn Bie na gu ba naa ka a dɛɛr sʋɔ kʋ̃ sɩɩr ba ɛ.
62005019	Sɩn bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka sɩ ɩn Nãaŋmɩn bibiir, ka a wɛr wʋ jaa be a dɛɛr sʋɔ tʋ̃ɔfʋ pɔ.
62005020	Sɩ mɩ bɔ̃ɔn naa ɩka Nãaŋmɩn Bie wa naa, 'lɔ lɛ vɛ̃ ka sɩ bɔ̃ɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ. Sɩ be naa a Nãaŋmɩn nyã nɩ a wʋ Bie Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ.
62005021	N bibiir, yɩ tɔɔ yɩ mɩ̃ɛ yin bʋtɩbɛ jaa pɔ.
63001001	Maa nɩkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ a fʋ̃ʋ pɔɔ nyã Nãaŋmɩn na ir nɩ a fʋ bibiir. N nʋ̃ fʋ naa nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ, a ba ɩ maa tɛɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ bala jaa mɩ na bɔ̃ɔ a yelmɩ̃ɛ mɩ nʋ̃ fʋ naa.
63001002	An ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ ben a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ jũu, na wʋn be a sɩ sɛ̃ sɔ̃ɔ jaa.
63001003	Wɩ̃ɛfʋ, nɩ nɩbaal, nɩ nyã'maar na yi a sɩ Sãa Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a wʋ Bie Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto a be a sɩn bala na be a yelmɩ̃ɛ nɩ a nʋ̃fʋ pɔ.
63001004	Nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ma naa ɩn nyɛ a fʋ bibiir bamɩne na chiine a yelmɩ̃ɛ pɔ, nɩtãa lɛ a Sãa na bin a nɛɛ kʋ sɩ.
63001005	Pʋ̃pãanyã n yɛpɔɔ, a ba ɩ nɛbin paalaa lɛ n sɛɛrɛ kʋrɔ fʋ ɛ, tɩchɛ a bʋ̃koraa 'lɔ lɛ na 'yɛr ɩka sɩ nʋ̃ taa.
63001006	A nʋ̃fʋ nɩ nyã ɩka sɩ turo a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na bin a wʋ nɛɛ kʋ sɩ. Wʋ 'yɛr ɩka sɩ nʋ̃ taa nɩtãa lɛ sɩn wõ yi a pielfʋ, sɩ ɩrɛ a lɛ nɛ.
63001007	Bɛ̃bɛlbɛ sɛɛn a wɛr, bala lɛ ba sɔɔ ɩka Yesu wan a wɛr pɔ nɩtãa nɩsaal ɛ. A nɩbɛ banyãna lɛ ɩ a bɛ̃bɛlbɛ tɩ 'laar a Kɩrɩsɩto.
63001008	Yɩ guro yɩ mɩ̃ɛ ka a yɩ tʋ̃mɔ̃ ta lo ɛ, tɩchɛ ka yɩ nyɛ a yɩ sãyar.
63001009	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na ba wa turo a lɛ a Yesu na wiil ɛ, waa tara nɛbʋ̃'yen nɩ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ, tɩ fʋ̃ʋ nyã na turo a lɛ wʋn wiil, tara naa Sãa nɩ a Bie.
63001010	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ wa wa naa a yɩ sɛ̃, tɩ ba tara a wiilfʋ nyã ɛ, yɩ ta sɔɔ ka wʋ kpɛ a yɩ yir bɩɩ puor wʋ ɛ.
63001011	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na puor a nɩnyɩnɛ nyãna mɩ pʋɔ naa a wʋ tʋ̃dɛɛr pɔ.
63001012	N chɛnɛ na tara yelyɔɔ ɩn taa sɛb kʋ fʋ, tɩchɛ ɩn bʋɔrɔ ɩka n wa a yɩ sɛ̃ jũu, maa wa wa sɩn 'mataa jɩ̃nɛ 'yɛrɛ ka nʋ̃ɔ nyɔɔ sɩ.
63001013	A yɛpɔɔ nyã mɩ a Nãaŋmɩn na ir bibiir mɩ puor fʋ naa.
64001001	Maa na ɩ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ sɛb a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a fʋ̃ʋ Gayus na ɩ a n baraa, ɩn nʋ̃ a yelmɩ̃ɛ jũu.
64001002	N baraa, n sʋɔrɔ na Nãaŋmɩn ɩka a fʋ ɩ̃gãn wʋ kpɛ̃mɛ ka a yele a jaa ɩ vɩla kʋ fʋ, nɩtãa lɛ a fʋ sɩɛ na kpɛ̃mɛ.
64001003	Nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ ma naa lɛ a yɛɛr bamɩne na wa 'yɛr a lɛ fʋn turo a yelmɩ̃ɛ na fʋ chiine a yelmɩ̃ɛ pɔ.
64001004	Bon jaa maa ɩ ma nʋ̃ɔ jɩ̃ ɩn maa wõ ɩka a n bibiir chiine naa a yelmɩ̃ɛ pɔ.
64001005	N baraa, fʋ tara na yelmɩ̃ɛ a lɛ fʋn maala kʋrɔ a yɛɛr, ba gba na ɩ sãanba a fʋ sɛ̃.
64001006	Ban wa, ba wa 'yɛr naa a fʋ nʋ̃fʋ kʋ a pupuorbiir a ka. Mɔ̃ na fʋ ma bar ba a sɔr a lɛ nɛ, lɛ lɛ pɛlɛ a Nãaŋmɩn pʋɔ.
64001007	Yesu yuor jũu lɛ ba chiine, na ba maa sɔɔ de bon jaa a bala na ba ɩ a Yesu turbo sɛ̃ ɛ.
64001008	Sɩn lɛ a sɛɛ ɩka sɩ sʋ̃ʋ ba na sɩ pʋɔ ba 'mataa tʋ̃ kʋ a yelmɩ̃ɛ.
64001009	N sɛb sɛbile kʋ a pupuorbiir na be a fʋ sɛ̃, tɩchɛ a Diotɩrefes na bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ ɩ a nɩdiere, sɩn nɩ 'lɔ ba tara nɛbʋ̃'yen ɛ.
64001010	Ala lɛ so, maa wa tɩ ɩn 'yɛr yɩ naa a lɛ wʋn yʋɔrɔ hũhũnõ ŋmara a jirsɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ sɩ. A lɛ tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ, tɩ wʋ maa sɔɔ de a sɩ yɛɛr ɛ. Wʋ ma ŋmaan a bala na bʋɔrɔ ɩka ba de ba sɔr tɩ ma dii ba bar a puorfʋ jie.
64001011	N baraa, ta tɔɔr yeldɛɛr ɛ, tɩchɛ tɔɔrɔ yelvɩla, nɩrɛ 'lɔ na maala vɩla bɔ̃ɔn Nãaŋmɩn. Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ 'lɔ mɩ na maala dɛɛr ba bɔ̃ɔ Nãaŋmɩn ɛ.
64001012	Demetirus, nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr a wʋ vɩla maalfʋ 'yɛr, a yelmɩ̃ɛ mɩ din a wʋ dãasɩɛ. Sɩn mɩ din a wʋ vɩla dãasɩɛ, ka yɩn mɩ bɔ̃ɔn ɩka a sɩ dãasɩɛ ɩn sɩrɛ.
64001013	N chɛnɛ na tara yelyɔɔ ɩn taa sɛb kʋ fʋ, tɩchɛ n ba bʋɔrɔ ɩka n sɛb ɛ.
64001014	A kʋ̃ lɛ kor ɛ, n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n nyɛ fʋ a sɩ jɩ̃nɛ 'yɛr.
64001015	Nyã'maar wʋ be a fʋ sɛ̃. A sɩ barmɩne na be ka puor fʋ naa, mɩ puor a sɩ barmɩne na be a be bʋ̃'yen 'yen.
65001001	Maa Judɩ na ɩ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto gbãgbaa, naa mɩ ɩ a Jemesɩ yɛbɛ, lɛ sɛɛrɛ a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a yɩn bala a Sãa Nãaŋmɩn na bʋɔl a yɩ be a wʋ nʋ̃fʋ pɔ ka wʋ gu yɩ taa lɛɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ.
65001002	Nɩbaal nɩ nyã'maar nɩ nʋ̃fʋ a dɔɔlɔ yɩ taa.
65001003	N barmɩne, n dɔ̃ɔ mʋ̃ɔ nɩbir ɩka n sɛb a faafʋ nyã sɩ jaa na põ, naa nyɛ ɩka a sɛɛ naa ka n sɛb kpãkpãan yɩ a yɩ mʋɔrɔ nɩ a sɔɔfʋ 'yɛr 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na de kʋ a wʋ nɩbɛ.
65001004	Nɩbɛ bamɩne sɔ̃ɔfʋ yele na dɔ̃ɔ sɛb bin kõr jaa sɔɔl naa na ba fʋɔl kpɛ a yɩ pɔ. Baa puoro ɛ, ba nyɔɔn a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn wɩ̃ɛfʋ yele lɩɛb na ba nyɛ sɔr sɛ̃nɛ tɩ na ba tɔr a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto tɛɛ na ɩ a sɩ Tʋ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a sɩ Soro.
65001005	Yɩ gba den nie bɔ̃ɔn a anyãna, tɩ n bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka n lɛ jɛɔ yɩ ɩka, a sɩ Soro faan a wʋ nɩbɛ yin a Ijipitɩ tẽe pɔ, tɩchɛ wʋ lɛ wa nyʋɔl a bala jaa na ba sɔɔ ɛ.
65001006	A malakasɩ bala na ba ara a ba tʋ̃ɔfʋ araa jie ɛ, tɩchɛ na ba tɔr a ba mɩ̃ɛ yir bar, bala lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn lũn a bɔ̃jɔr kpɩ̃ɛn 'yɔ̃ɔ be a libe pɔ chɛlɛ nɩ a 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ bɩbir kpɛ̃ɛ daar.
65001007	A lɛ nɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, a Sodom nɩ a Gomora, nɩ a tẽchɛɛlsɩ ala na jilʋ̃ de a ba mɩ̃ɛ kʋ a sɛ̃sɛ̃yele, ka dɔɔr gãna nɩ taa, ka a bũu na ba kpĩine ɛ, di ba, naa ɩ yelmanaa gã.
65001008	A lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ, a jãna dẽme banyãna sɔ̃ɔn a ba ɩ̃gãma, baa turo a sɩ Soro binfʋ ɛ. Ba ma kpɛrɛ naa a saaju bʋ̃maalsɩ.
65001009	Tɩchɛ a Maɩkɩl gba na ɩ a malakasɩ nɩkpɛ̃ɛ a 'lɔ naa Tɩɩ na dɔ̃ɔ chɩrɛ taa nɩ Mosesɩ ɩ̃gãn yele, waa 'la tu a Tɩɩ bɩɩ kpɛ wʋ ɛ, tɩ na wʋ 'yɛr, "A sɩ Soro lɛ na kpãa fʋ."
65001010	Tɩchɛ a nɩbɛ banyãna ma kpɛrɛ naa a bonsɩ ala ban ba bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, ka a yelsɩ ala ban ba bɔ̃ɔ yi a ba dɔɔfʋ daar, kaara fɩka dʋ̃n na ba tara tɩɛr ɛ, a yelsɩ anyãna lɛ na sɔ̃ɔ ba.
65001011	Nɛbier nyɔɔ ba naa, bojũu ba den a Kain sɔr. Tɔ̃nɔ̃ jũu a ba far kpɛ a Balaam bɔrfʋ pɔ. A nɛchɩrɛ jũu, ba mɩ nyʋɔl naa a Kora kaar.
65001012	A nɩbɛ banyãna kaara fɩka bʋ̃sɔ̃ɔnsɩ na jɛr yɩ a yɩ nɛbʋ̃'yen lɔ̃ɔ di daar. Ba maa bɛɛ nɩrɛ ɛ, ba mɩ̃ɛ lɛ ba kaara. Ba ɩn julõjuur na ba tara kʋ̃ɔ ɛ, ka a sɛsɛbɛ furo yʋɔrɔ nɩ. Ba kaara fɩka kpãchãan tɩɩr na ba tara wɔ̃mɔ̃ ɛ, ka ba vɔ̃ dɩɛl bar ka a kpi.
65001013	Ba kaara na fɩka a man kpɛ̃ɛ a sɛsɛkpɛ̃ɛ na furo ka a ba vɩ̃ furo a kʋ̃ɔ fuul kaar, na ba kaara fɩka ŋmarbie bɔrɔ yʋɔrɔ ka a Nãaŋmɩn chɔɔr jilibe jaa gbɛb guro nɩ ba.
65001014	Enok na ɩ a Adama yɔ̃ɔ suulaa ayopõi sʋɔ mɩ dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr a nɩbɛ banyãna 'yɛr, "Nyɛ, a sɩ Soro waara naa nɩ a wʋ nɩchɛchɛsɩ turo turo.
65001015	Wʋn wa tɔɔr nɩrɛ jaa 'yɛr, na wʋ 'yɛr a lɛ a bala na ba puoro ɛ, a lɛ jaa ban tʋ̃ nɩ a lɛ ban maal tɔr a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a 'yɛr bikpɩ̃ɛn ala ban 'yɛr dɔɔl wʋ."
65001016	A nɩbɛ banyãna lɛ ma ɩrɛ gbʋrɔ̃ gbʋrɔ̃, na ba nyɛrɛ a ba taaba bɔrfʋ. Ba ma turo naa a ba mɩ̃ɛ vɔldɛɛr, a ba mɩ̃ɛ yobɔ 'yɛr lɛ ba ma 'yɛrɛ bɛlɛ nɩ a ba taaba tɔ̃nɔ̃ jũu.
65001017	Tɩchɛ n barmɩne, yɩ tɩɛr a lɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩtʋ̃nsɩ na dɔ̃ɔ 'yɛr.
65001018	Ba 'yɛr kʋ yɩ ɩka, "A ber baaraa sɔ̃ɔ, nɩlaarba na turo a ba ɩ̃gãn vɔlaa na wa naa."
65001019	A nɩbɛ banyãna lɛ ma waan ootaa, na ba turo a ɩ̃gãn bɔfʋ na baa tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ɛ.
65001020	Tɩchɛ a yɩn n barmɩne, yɩ mɛ a yɩ mɩ̃ɛ dɔɔl a yɩ sɔɔfʋ chɛchɛ ju, na yɩ sʋɔrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a wʋ Sɩɛ kpɛ̃ɔ.
65001021	Yɩ sɔɔl yɩ mɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nʋ̃fʋ pɔ na yɩ chɛlɛ a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto nɩbaal, a wʋ waan a nyɛvʋr na ba tara baarfʋ ɛ, wa kʋ yɩ.
65001022	Yɩ tara a bala na baala nɩ nɩbaal.
65001023	Yɩ vʋ̃ɔ a bamɩne yin a bũu pɔ na yɩ faa ba. Na yɩ mɩ kaa a bamɩne nɩbaal tɩ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ jʋ̃mɔ̃, na yɩ taa maal a ba dɛɛr ala ban maala ɛ.
65001024	A 'lɔ na gu yɩ ka yɩ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ lo ɛ, na wʋn wa waan yɩ a wʋ tɩɩr niem a yɩ kʋ̃ tara chɛfʋ ɛ, ka a nʋ̃ɔ kpɛ̃ɛ kpɛ yɩ.
65001025	A Nãaŋmɩn bʋ̃'yen nyã tɛɛ lɛ ɩ a sɩ Fafaara, wʋ nyɛ tɩɩr, nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ, nɩ tʋ̃ɔfʋ tu a sɩ Soro Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto 'yɔ̃ɔ sɛrɛ tɩ wʋ wa maal a wɛr nɩ pʋ̃pãanyã bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa! A ɩ a lɛ.
66001001	A yelwiilsɩ ala a Nãaŋmɩn na kʋ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto ɩka wʋ wiil kʋ a wʋ gbãgbaa ala kʋ̃ yaar tɩ ɩ ɛ. Yesu tʋ̃ naa a wʋ malaka ɩka wʋ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ a wʋ gbãgbaa Jɔɔn.
66001002	Jɔɔn mɩ man naa a ala a jaa wʋn nyɛ na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nɩ lɛ a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto na 'yɛr.
66001003	Pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ na kar a gãn nyã. Pʋpɛl dẽme mɩ lɛ a bala na wõ tɩ de 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba nyãn pɔ, lɛ an sɛb a gãn nyã pɔ, bojũu a bɩbir gbʋr naa.
66001004	Maa Jɔɔn lɛ sɛb a gãn nyã kʋrɔ a yɩn pupuorbiir gbulsɩ ayopõi na be Asɩya paal pɔ. Wɩ̃ɛfʋ nɩ nyã'maar yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ, 'lɔ lɛ be be, nɩ 'lɔ lɛ na wa, naa yi a Sɩɩr ayopõi na ara a Nãaŋmɩn dakɔɔ niem,
66001005	naa yi a Yesu Kɩrɩsɩto sɛ̃, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ dãasɩɛ sʋɔ, na wʋ ɩ a bidɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ na ir a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋr, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a nãmɩne ba jaa nãkpɛ̃ɛ na be ka a wɛr pɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ nʋ̃ sɩ na wʋ de a wʋ jɩ̃ɩ pɛɛ sɩ yin a sɩ yeldɛɛr pɔ na wʋ faa sɩ,
66001006	na wʋ maal sɩ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ nɩbɛ nɩ Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lorbo ka sɩn tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a wʋ Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a Sãa, 'lɔ lɛ so a tɩɩr nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ a bɩbir nɩ bɩbir jaa! A ɩ a lɛ.
66001007	Yɩ nyɛ, wʋn yi naa a sajulõjuur pɔ waara, ka a nɩbɛ ba jaa nyɛ wʋ lɔ̃ɔn a bala na chɔr wʋ, a nɩbʋrsɩ na be ka a tẽe na kõnõ naa a wʋ waa jũu. Lɛ lɛ an ɩ! A ɩ a lɛ.
66001008	A sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ jaa sʋɔ 'yɛr naa, "Maa lɛ a Pielfʋ nɩ a Baaraa. Maa lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be. Maa lɛ chɛnɛ be be. Maa lɛ na wa."
66001009	Maa Jɔɔn na ɩ a yɩ yɛbɛ, n pʋɔ yɩ naa a dɔɔyɛ pɔ a Yesu tufʋ jũu. Maa nɩ yɩn jaa ben a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ tɩ chɛnɛ tara kãnyir. N ben a man dõdol pɔ ban bʋɔlɔ Patimosɩ bojũu n 'yɛr naa a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr naa di a Yesu dãasɩɛ.
66001010	A sɩ Soro Bɩbir Daar, Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ ir ma naa ka n wõ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ na tãn a n puor fɩka ɩɩl ban pɛɛl,
66001011	ka a kɔkɔr 'yɛr, "Sɛb a ala a jaa fʋn nyɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ a gãn pɔ, na fʋ tɩr kʋ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ ayopõi. Efesus, Semena, Pergamum, Tayatira, Saadisɩ, Feladelfiya nɩ Laodisea."
66001012	N lɩɛb ɩka n kaa an lɛ 'yɛrɛ a lɛ kʋrɔ ma. Ɩn wa lɩɛb, n nyɛn sɛlma fɩ̃tɩnɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie jiir ayopõi.
66001013	A fɩ̃tɩnɛ dɔɔlfʋ jiir anyãna sãlsɔɔ, n nyɛn nɩrɛ na kaara fɩka Nɩsaal Bie na wʋ su fuu wõo ka wʋ ta a gbɛɛ pɔ, tɩ a sɛlma gãn bãbɩ̃ a wʋ nyãa ju.
66001014	A wʋ jukɔɔl pɛl fɩka gõn, ka a nɩbie kaara fɩka bũu na 'lɩrɛ.
66001015	Ka a gbɛɛ nyɩlɛ fɩka kur jɩɛ ban juu ir sãa pɔ, ka a kɔkɔr wʋn 'yɛrɛ nyɛtãan kɔ̃kpɛ̃ɛ na joro.
66001016	Ŋmɛrbie ayopõi be naa a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ pɔ, ka a sɔbʋraa na dire a jiir a jaa ayi, yi a wʋ nɛɛ pɔ. Ka a wʋ nie nyɩlɛ fɩka mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ na ara gar ju sãlsɔɔ.
66001017	Ɩ̃n wa nyɛ a lɛ, ka n lo kpa a wʋ niem gã fɩka kũu. Ka wʋ pãa dɔɔl ma a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ tɩ 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Ta joro dãbɩ̃ɛ ɛ. Maa lɛ a Pielfʋ nɩ a Baaraa.
66001018	Maa lɛ ɩ a Nyɛvʋr Sʋɔ. Nyɛ, n dɔ̃ɔ kpi, tɩchɛ n ir naa ɩ vʋr, n kʋ̃ lɛ kpi go ɛ. Maa lɛ tara a kũu nɩ a kpĩisɩ tẽe pãn bir.
66001019	"A lɛ juu sɛb a ala fʋn nyɛ na dɔ̃ɔ ɩ nɩ a pʋ̃pãanyã, nɩ a ala na wa ɩ daar kɔ̃ɔ.
66001020	A yelsɔɔlaa 'lɔ na be a ŋmɛrbie ayopõi ala fʋn nyɛ a n nũsʋ̃ɔ pɔ nɩ a sɛlma fɩ̃tɩnɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie jiir ayopõi par nɩ nyã. A ŋmɛrbie ayopõi ala ɩ naa a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ ayopõi malakasɩ, fɩ̃tɩnɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie jiir ayopõi mɩ ɩ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ ayopõi.
66002001	"Sɛb kʋ a malaka 'lɔ na ara kʋ a Efesus pupuorbiir ɩka, a 'lɔ na tara a ŋmɛrbie ayopõi a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ pɔ na wʋ chiine a sɛlma fɩ̃tɩnɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie jiir ayopõi sãlsɔɔ 'yɛr lɛ a anyãna.
66002002	N bɔ̃ɔ naa a lɛ fʋn be, naa bɔ̃ɔ a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ nɩ a fʋ kãnyir. N bɔ̃ɔn naa a lɛ fʋn ba 'maa nɩbir kʋ a putudẽme ɛ, ala lɛ so ka fʋ bɛɛr a bala na 'yɛr ɩka Yesu nɩtʋ̃nsɩ lɛ ba ɩ na fʋ nyɛ ka ba ɩ jir ŋmarba.
66002003	Fʋ tara na kãnyir na fʋ di dɔɔyɛ a n yuor jũu, tɩ faa bal ɛ.
66002004	Tɩchɛ n chɛnɛ na tara fʋ nɩ 'yɛr. Fʋ bar naa a fʋ dɔ̃ɔ nʋ̃fʋ 'lɔ.
66002005	Tɩɛr kaa a lɛ fʋn dɔ̃ɔ be tɩ wa lo! Lɩɛb a fʋ tɩɛr na fʋ be a lɛ fʋn dɔ̃ɔ be. Ala ɩ fʋ̃ʋ ba wa lɩɛb a fʋ tɩɛr ɛ, ɩn wa naa wa 'lɔɔ a fʋ fɩ̃tɩn dɔɔlfʋ jie bar.
66002006	Tɩchɛ a lɛ fʋn ba nʋ̃ nɩ nyã, fʋ 'laar naa a Nikolayitɩ nɩbɛ maalfʋ, n mɩ 'laar naa a ba maalfʋ.
66002007	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor wʋ chɛlɛ a ala a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ. A 'lɔ na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ, ɩn kʋ wʋn sɔr ka wʋ kpɛ a Nãaŋmɩn jɔɔ pɔ pɔr a nyɛvʋr tɩɛ wɔ̃mɔ̃ na wʋ di.
66002008	"Sɛb kʋ a malaka 'lɔ na ara kʋ a Semena pupuorbiir ɩka, a 'lɔ na ɩ a Pielfʋ nɩ a Baaraa, a 'lɔ na kpi tɩ ir ɩ vʋr 'yɛr lɛ a anyãna.
66002009	N bɔ̃ɔ naa a fʋ wõm nɩ a fʋ nɔ̃ɔ tɩchɛ fʋ ɩn taraa sʋɔ! N bɔ̃ɔ naa a gagarsɩ bala na 'yɛr ɩka Juu nɩbɛ lɛ ba ɩ tɩ na baa ɩ ɛ, ba ɩ naa Satan lɔ̃ɔfʋ dẽme.
66002010	Taa joro dãbɩ̃ɛ a dɔɔyɛ na wa a fʋ sɛ̃ ɛ. Nyɛ, a tɩɩ na vɛ̃ naa ka ba nyɔɔr a yɩ bamɩne 'yɔ̃ɔ pɔɔfʋ die pɔ, bɛɛr yɩ kaa, ka yɩ di dɔɔyɛ ber pie. Ala ɩ yɩn kpin gba, yɩ taa bara a yɩ sɔɔfʋ ɛ, ka ɩn kʋ yɩ a nyɛvʋr 'lɔ na kaara a nãa jupil kaar.
66002011	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor wʋ chɛlɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ. Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ, a gbɛɛ ayi kũu kʋ̃ lɛ sɩɩr wʋ go ɛ.
66002012	"Sɛb kʋ a malaka 'lɔ na ara kʋ a Pergamum pupuorbiir ɩka, a 'lɔ a sɔbʋraa na dire a jiir a jaa ayi 'yɛr lɛ anyãna.
66002013	N bɔ̃ɔ naa a jie fʋn kpɩɛrɛ, be lɛ ɩ a Satan dʋʋ, tɩ faa vɛ̃ a n yuor bʋɔlfʋ ɛ. Fʋ chɛnɛ na sɔɔ a n yuor. Fʋ gba na wa nyɛ a Antipasɩ na dire a n dãasɩɛ ka ba kʋ wʋ a yɩ tẽe pɔ be a Satan dʋʋ na be.
66002014	Tɩchɛ n chɛnɛ na tara fʋ nɩ 'yɛr. Fʋ chɛnɛ na tara nɩbɛ ka ba turo a Balaam wiilfʋ, 'lɔ lɛ wiil a Balak ɩka wʋ bɛr a Isɩral nɩbɛ nɛɛ ka ba maal dɛɛr na wʋ ɩka ba di a bʋtɩbɛ bʋ̃diir na ba gãna nɩ taa.
66002015	A lɛ nɩ wʋ ju mɩ lɛ fʋ mɩ chɛnɛ tara a nɩbɛ na turo a Nikolayitɩ nɩbɛ wiilfʋ.
66002016	Lɩɛb a fʋ tɩɛr, ka lɛ ba lɛ ɛ, ɩn wan fɔɔ wa jɛb a nɩbɛ bala nɩ a sɔbʋraa 'lɔ na yi a n nɛɛ pɔ.
66002017	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor, wʋ chɛlɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ. A 'lɔ na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ, ɩn kʋ wʋn a maana ala na sɔɔl. Naa lɛ kʋ wʋ kusɩr pɩla ban sɛb yopaalaa dɔɔl nɩrɛ jaa na ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, a 'lɔ na so lɛ bɔ̃ɔ.
66002018	"Sɛb kʋ a malaka 'lɔ na ara kʋ a Tayatira pupuorbiir ɩka, a Nãaŋmɩn Bie 'yɛr lɛ a anyãna. A 'lɔ nɩbie na kaara a bũu 'lɩraa kaar ka a wʋ gbɛɛ nyɛtãan fɩka kur jɩɛ na be bũu pɔ.
66002019	N bɔ̃ɔ naa a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃, a fʋ nʋ̃fʋ, a fʋ sɔɔfʋ nɩ a fʋ kãnyir. A lɛ fʋn tʋ̃nɔ̃ a pʋ̃pãanyã gar a lɛ fʋn dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃.
66002020	Tɩchɛ n chɛnɛ na tara fʋ nɩ 'yɛr. Fʋ bal kʋ a pɔɔ 'lɔ ban bʋɔlɔ a Jejebɛl 'lɔ na bʋɔlɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛ'yɛrɛ. Wʋ wile naa a n tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ ka ba sɛ̃nɛ na ba ɔɔrɔ nɩ a bʋtɩbɛ nʋ̃nɔ̃.
66002021	N kʋ wʋn sɔ̃ɔ ɩka wʋ lɩɛb a wʋ tɩɛr yin a wʋ sɛ̃sɛ̃yele pɔ, tɩchɛ waa sɔɔrɔ ɛ.
66002022	Lɛ ɩn vɛ̃n ka baal nyɔɔ wʋ ka bala naa 'lɔ na sɛ̃nɛ, ka bala baa lɩɛb bar a wʋ sɔr ɛ.
66002023	Ɩn kʋ naa a bala na turo wʋ, ka a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ bɔ̃ɔ ɩka maa lɛ bɔ̃ɔ nɩrɛ tɩɛr nɩ nɩrɛ nyãa naa na yab ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa nɩ wʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃.
66002024	Tɩchɛ a yɩn na chɛ a be a Tayatira na ba de a pɔɔ wiilfʋ bɩɩ jãn a Satan yelsɔɔlsɩ ɛ, n chɛnɛ na tara 'yɛr na 'yɛr kʋ yɩ. N kʋ̃ de yele jaa dɔɔl yɩ ɛ.
66002025	Yɩ chɛnɛ nyɔɔ a lɛ nɛ wa tãn a daar 'lɔ ɩn na wa.
66002026	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ na wʋ ɩrɛ a lɛ ɩn bʋɔrɔ, ɩn kʋ wʋn kpɛ̃ɔ ka wʋ tʋ̃ɔ a paalsɩ ba jaa,
66002027	'Wʋn kaara ba naa nɩ kur dãgbal na wʋ ma ŋmɛr ba lamɩɛr kaar.' Nɩtãa lɛ ɩn nyɛ a kpɛ̃ɔ yin a n Sãa sɛ̃.
66002028	N mɩ na kʋ wʋ naa a bivɩɛ ŋmɛrbir.
66002029	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor wʋ chɛlɛ a ala Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ.
66003001	"Sɛb kʋ a malaka 'lɔ na ara kʋ a Saadisɩ pupuorbiir ɩka, a 'lɔ na tara a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɩr ayopõi nɩ a ŋmɛrbie ayopõi, n bɔ̃ɔ naa a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃. A fʋ yuor yire na ɩka fʋ ɩn bʋ̃vʋr tɩchɛ bʋ̃kũu lɛ fʋ ɩ.
66003002	Jɛɔ ir! Na fʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ a bala na chɛ na kpire ɩ̃kpɩ̃ɛn, bojũu n jʋʋr nyɛ ka a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ ba sɛɛ a n Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ɛ.
66003003	Tɩɛr tɔ a ala fʋn de tɩ wõ, turo a ala tɩ na fʋ lɩɛb a tɩɛr. Tɩchɛ fʋ̃ʋ ba jɛɔ ir ɛ, ɩn wan nãnyie kaar ka fʋ kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔ a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn na wa a fʋ sɛ̃ ɛ.
66003004	Tɩchɛ fʋ chɛnɛ na tara nɩbɛ bɩ̃lãa a ba be a Saadisɩ ka a ba fɔɔr ba nyɔɔr dɛbɛ ɛ. Bala nɩ maa na 'mantaa chiine, ka ba su bʋ̃pɩɛl, bojũu ba sɛɛn naa.
66003005	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ a ba kaar mɩ na sun a bʋ̃pɩɛl. N kʋ̃ kpĩin a wʋ yuor bar a nyɛvʋr gãn pɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ ɩn pʋr a wʋ yuor a n Sãa nɩ a wʋ malakasɩ niem.
66003006	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor, wʋ chɛlɛ a ala a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ.
66003007	"Sɛb kʋ a malaka 'lɔ na ara kʋ a Feladelfiya pupuorbiir ɩka, a 'lɔ na ɩ a chɛchɛ sʋɔ nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ 'yɛr lɛ a anyã, 'lɔ lɛ tara a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ David pãn bir. 'Lɔ wa yuo, nɩrɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ pɔɔ ɛ, 'lɔ mɩ wa pɔɔ, nɩrɛ kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ yuo ɛ.
66003008	N bɔ̃ɔ naa a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ a jaa. Nyɛ, n yuo naa a pãn bar, nɩrɛ jaa na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ pɔɔ ɛ. N bɔ̃ɔ naa a fʋ kpɛ̃ɔ na ba jɩ̃ bon ɛ, tɩchɛ fʋ chɛnɛ na tara a n 'yɛr na faa chiir a n yuor ɛ.
66003009	N bɔ̃ɔ naa a bala na ɩ a Satan lɔ̃ɔfʋ dẽme tɩ na ba 'yɛr ɩka Juu nɩbɛ lɛ ba ɩ, jir ŋmarba lɛ ba ɩ. Ɩn vɛ̃ naa ka ba wa gbur dumo a yɩ niem na ba bɔ̃ɔ ɩka n nʋ̃ yɩ naa.
66003010	A lɛ fʋn tu a n 'yɛr na fʋ di kãnyir, ɩn gu fʋ naa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ a dɔɔyɛ na wa a nɩbɛ ba jaa jie na kpɩɛrɛ ka a wɛr pɔ.
66003011	N kʋ̃ kor tɩ wa ɛ. Nyɔɔ a lɛ nɛ fʋn tara, ka nɩrɛ jaa taa faa a fʋ nãa jupil ɛ.
66003012	A 'lɔ na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ, ɩn maal wʋn a luur a n Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir. Wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ vʋ̃ɔ go ɛ. Ɩn sɛb naa a n Nãaŋmɩn yuor nɩ a n Nãaŋmɩn tẽe yuor na ɩ a Jerusalɛm paalaa wʋn bar ka wʋ yire a saaju suro waara mar wʋ, naa mɩ lɛ sɛb a n yopaalaa mar wʋ.
66003013	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor, wʋ chɛlɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ.
66003014	"Sɛb kʋ a malaka 'lɔ na ara kʋ a Laodisea pupuorbiir ɩka, a 'lɔ 'yɛrbie na ɩ A Ɩ A Lɛ, a yelmɩ̃ɛ dẽ dẽ sʋɔ nɩ a yelmɩ̃ɛ dãasɩɛ sʋɔ, 'lɔ 'yɔ̃ɔ lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn tu mɛ bomo a jaa.
66003015	N bɔ̃ɔ naa a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃, faa 'maa ɛ, faa lɛ tʋlɔ mɩ ɛ. An taa nʋ̃mɔ̃ ma naa ala ɩ fʋ ta 'maa naa bɩɩ tʋlɔ.
66003016	A lɛ fʋn ben ɩ a ʋlɔ ʋlɔ jũu, faa tʋlɔ ɛ, faa mɩ lɛ 'maa ɛ, ɩn chɩr fʋn bar a n nɛɛ pɔ.
66003017	Fʋ 'yɛr ɩka taraa sʋɔ lɛ fʋ ɩ, na fʋ tara nãbonsɩ na faa faa bon jaa ɛ. Tɩchɛ faa bɔ̃ɔ ɩka fʋ ɩn nɩkɔ̃ɔ nɩ nɩbaal nɩrɛ, nɩ nɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ, na fʋ ɩ jɔ̃ɔ nɩ sal'mʋɔr.
66003018	N sʋɔrɔ fʋ naa ɩka fʋ da sɛlma a n sɛ̃ ɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ bũu pɔ maal na fʋ ɩ tara sʋɔ. Na fʋ mɩ da fɔpɩla a n sɛ̃ pɔɔ a fʋ sal'mʋɔr vĩ, na fʋ lɛ da a nɩbie tɩ̃ɩ mɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a nɩbie pɔ nyɛrɛ.
66003019	N ma gɔ̃ naa a bala ɩn nʋ̃, naa tɔɔ ba toor. A lɛ mɔ̃ nɩbijɩɛ lɩɛb a fʋ tɩɛr.
66003020	Nyɛ, n ara naa dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ bʋɔlɔ, ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa wõ naa a n kɔkɔr na wʋ yuo a pãn, ɩn kpɛ naa ka a maa naa nɩnyɩnɛ a sɩ tɩ 'mataa dire.
66003021	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ, ɩn kʋ wʋn sɔr ka wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a n lõboor nɩtãa lɛ ɩn jɛb tʋ̃ɔ naa jɩ̃nɛ a n Sãa lõboor.
66003022	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor, wʋ chɛlɛ a lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ na 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ."
66004001	A anyã puor, n lɛ kãan nyɛ a saaju pãn na yuo ara. Ka a kɔkɔr 'lɔ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ wõ a ɩɩl ban pɛɛl kaar 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Do wa, ka n wiil fʋ a ala na ɩ a anyã puor."
66004002	Ajienaa kaa ɩ Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ de ma naa ka n nyɛ a nãa dakɔɔ a be a saaju nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ na jɩ̃nɛ.
66004003	Ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju nyɩlɛ jaa pala pala fɩka gar kʋsɩr, nɩ kʋsɩr wolo wolo, ka a sagõgoraa na nyɩlɛ ŋmaa jilʋ̃ a nãa dakɔɔ.
66004004	Dakɔɔr lɩjɛr nɩ anaar mɩ ben be jilʋ̃ a nãa dakɔɔ, ka a nɩbɛrɛ lɩjɛr nɩ anaar mɩ jɩ̃nɛ a ju, na ba su bʋ̃pɩɛl na ba sun sɛlma jupile.
66004005	Saa nyɩɩrfʋ nɩ gɔ̃mɔ̃ na tãna yire naa a nãa dakɔɔ par. Ka a fɩ̃tɩnɛ ayopõi mɩ 'lɩrɛ a nãa dakɔɔ par, anyãna lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɩr ayopõi.
66004006	A nãa dakɔɔ niem bon ben be kaara man kʋ̃ɔ kaar jaa wel wel wel, na wʋ nyɩlɛ chãana kaar. A bʋ̃nɩbie anaar jil naa a nãa dakɔɔ tara nɩbie a jiir a jaa a puor nɩ a niem.
66004007	A bʋ̃nɩbir 'lɔ na de nie nyɛtãan jukpɛ̃ɛ, ka a ayi sʋɔ mɩ nyɛtãan narbile, ka a ata sʋɔ mɩ nyɛtãan nɩsaal, ka a anaar sʋɔ mɩ nyɛtãan tuu.
66004008	A bʋ̃nɩbie anyãna ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tara naa pɩbɛ ayʋɔb, ka a nɩbie pɔɔ a ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa naa pɩbɛ pɔ. Ba ma yiele nɩ yiel mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ ɩka, "Chɛchɛ, chɛchɛ, chɛchɛ 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ jaa sʋɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ be be, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ, 'lɔ lɛ na wa."
66004009	Sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jaa a bʋ̃nɩbie ala na ma wa puoro pɛɛrɛ dãna nɩ a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju, 'lɔ lɛ be be jaa kpo kpo,
66004010	a nɩbɛrɛ lɩjɛr nɩ anaar bala gãn kpa tẽe tɩ puor a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju, 'lɔ lɛ na be be jaa kpo kpo. Ba yãan a ba nãjupile bin a nãa dakɔɔ par tɩ 'yɛrɛ,
66004011	"A sɩ Soro nɩ a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ a sɛɛn ɩka fʋ de a tɩɩr, 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ. Bojũu fʋ̃ʋ lɛ maal a bomo a jaa, a fʋ bɔfʋ pɔ lɛ a jaa maal naa be be."
66005001	N pãa nyɛn a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju ka wʋ tara a kõr gãn 'lɔ ban pilʋ̃ a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ pɔ, ka a sɛbie be a pʋɔ pɔ nɩ a yõo, na ba de jɩ̃nsɩ ayopõi mar pɔɔ.
66005002	N nyɛn a malaka kpɛ̃ɔ sʋɔ 'lɔ na de nɛkpɛ̃ɛ sʋʋr, "An lɛ sɛɛ ɩka wʋ 'lɔɔr a jɩ̃nsɩ tɩ yuo a gãn?"
66005003	Tɩchɛ nɩrɛ jaa ba be a saaju, bɩɩ a wɛr pɔ, bɩɩ a tẽe par na tʋ̃ɔ yuo a gãn kar ɛ.
66005004	Ka n kõ nɩbaal kõn bojũu nɩrɛ jaa na ba be be sɛɛn na yuo a gãn kar kaa ɛ.
66005005	Be lɛ a nɩbɛrɛ bala ɩ̃sʋɔ pãa 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Ta kõnõ ɛ. Nyɛ a Jukpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ na yi a Juda bʋrɔ pɔ, na ɩ a Nãkpɛ̃ɛ David yɔ̃ɔ na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ. 'Lɔ lɛ sɛɛ na tʋ̃ɔ 'lɔɔr a jɩ̃nsɩ ala bar tɩ yuo a gãn."
66005006	N pãa lɛ nyɛn Pɛraabile ka wʋ nyɛtãan bon ban dɔ̃ɔ kʋ ka wʋ ara a nãa dakɔɔ par, ka a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ ara jilʋ̃ wʋ. Wʋ tara na ɩlɛ ayopõi nɩ nɩbie ayopõi, ala lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɩr ayopõi wʋn ma tʋ̃ a wɛr pɔ jiir a jaa.
66005007	'Lɔ lɛ tɩ de a gãn a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju nũsʋ̃ɔ pɔ.
66005008	Wʋn wa de a gãn ka a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ lɩjɛr nɩ anaar bala, ba jaa gãn kpa tẽe a Pɛraabile niem, ka ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tara kõrõjom nɩ sɛlma lapʋɛ na sɛɛn a tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla, ala lɛ ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ sʋɔrfʋsɩ.
66005009	Bala lɛ yiele a yiel paalaa na ba 'yɛrɛ, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ sɛɛn ɩka fʋ de a gãn na fʋ 'lɔɔr a jɩ̃nsɩ, bojũu fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ba kʋ, ka fʋ de a fʋ jɩ̃ɩ yab den nɩbʋrɔ, 'yɛr bʋrɔ, balsɩ ba jaa nɩ a paalsɩ a jaa kʋ Nãaŋmɩn.
66005010	Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ maal ba ka ba ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nãalʋ̃ʋ nɩbɛ nɩ a bɔɔrlorbo tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn, bala lɛ na wa ɩ a wɛr nyã wʋ jaa nãmɩne."
66005011	Be lɛ n pãa kaa nyɛ malakasɩ turo turo fʋn kʋ̃ bɔ̃ɔ a ba nɛɛ ɛ, ka ba ara jilʋ̃ a nãa dakɔɔ nɩ a bʋ̃nɩbie ala nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ bala.
66005012	Ba yiele naa nɩ kɔkɔkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛrɛ, "A Pɛraabile 'lɔ ban dɔ̃ɔ kʋ lɛ sɛɛn ɩka wʋ tara a kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ a nãbomo, nɩ a yɛ̃, nɩ a fɔ̃ɔ, nɩ a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, nɩ a tɩɩr, nɩ a dãnfʋ."
66005013	Be lɛ n wõ a bʋ̃maalsɩ a jaa na be a saaju, nɩ a tẽe, nɩ a tẽe par, nɩ a man pɔ, nɩ bomo a jaa na be a ba pɔ, na ba yiele yiel 'yɛrɛ, "A 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju, nɩ a Pɛraabile lɛ so a dãnfʋ, nɩ a 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, nɩ a tɩɩr, nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ, bɩbir jaa."
66005014	Ka a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala 'yɛr, "A ɩ a lɛ," ka a nɩbɛrɛ bala gbur dumo puor a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju nɩ a Pɛraabile.
66006001	Ka n kaa naa nyɛ a Pɛraabile na 'lɔɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ ayopõi ala ban mar a gãn 'lɔ na de nie, be lɛ n wõ a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala ɩ̃sʋɔ kɔkɔr fɩka saa na tãn, ka wʋ bʋɔl, "Wa!"
66006002	Be lɛ n kaa nyɛ ka a ɩ wii pɩla lɛ, ka a 'lɔ na do, jã tam a ba de nãa jupil kʋ wʋ ka wʋ yin darfʋ an ɩ tʋ̃ɔfʋ sʋɔ lɛ wʋ ɩ.
66006003	A Pɛraabile na lɛ 'lɔɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ ayi sʋ̃ɔ, n wõn a bʋ̃nɩbie ala ayi sʋɔ na 'yɛr, "Wa!"
66006004	Ka a wii jɩɛ wa yi, a 'lɔ na do ba kʋ wʋn kpɛ̃ɔ ɩka wʋ faa a nyã'maar tɩ vɛ̃ ka jɛɛr ir a wɛr wʋ jaa, ka a nɩbɛ kʋrɔ taa. Ka ba kʋ wʋ a jɛɛr sɔkpɛ̃ɛ.
66006005	A Pɛraabile na lɛ 'lɔɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ ata sʋɔ, n wõn a bʋ̃nɩbie ata sʋɔ na 'yɛr, "Wa!" Ka n kaa ka a ɩ wii sɔɔlaa lɛ, ka a 'lɔ na do tara bʋ̃mansɩ a nũu pɔ.
66006006	Be lɛ n wõ a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala chara pɔ fɩka kɔkɔr na 'yɛrɛ, "Kɔ̃ lo naa, chi bʋ̃manãa nɛbʋ̃'yen na da naa nɩbʋ̃'yen bɩbir gbul sãyar. Ka a kamaana mɩ nɛɛr ata mɩ da nɩbʋ̃'yen bɩbir gbul sãyar, tɩ taa ɩrɛ wa sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a kãa nɩ a dãa bara ɛ."
66006007	A Pɛraabile na lɛ 'lɔɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ anaar sʋɔ, n wõ naa a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar sʋɔ na 'yɛr, "Wa!"
66006008	Ka n kaa nyɛ wii ul a nɩdaa. Ka a 'lɔ na do yuor di kũu, ka a kpĩisɩ tẽe mɩ turo a wʋ puor. Ba kʋ ban kpɛ̃ɔ ɩka ba de sɔkpɛ̃ɛ, nɩ kɔ̃, nɩ baal, nɩ mɔdʋ̃n kʋn a wɛr nɩbɛ ala ɩ ba põn a tẽe a wʋ jiir anaar.
66006009	Wʋn lɛ 'lɔɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ anũu sʋɔ, n nyɛn a nɩsɩɩr bala ban dɔ̃ɔ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr nɩ a wʋ dãasɩɛ jũu ka ba be a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lofʋ jie pĩlem.
66006010	Ba tãna naa nɩ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛrɛ, "A Tʋ̃ɔfʋ sʋɔ, nɩ chɛchɛ sʋɔ, nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, a wa ta dabor ka fʋ tɔɔr a wɛr nɩbɛ 'yɛr na fʋ yab a sɩ jɩ̃ɩ sãma?"
66006011	Be lɛ ba kʋ ba jaa bʋ̃pɩɛl tɩ 'yɛr ɩka ba di kãnyir bɩ̃lãa ka ba baar kʋ a ba tʋ̃tʋ̃taaba nɩ a yɛɛr a ba kaar ka a ta.
66006012	N kaara naa ka wʋ lɛ 'lɔɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ ayʋɔb sʋɔ. Ka a tẽe mĩi wʋ jaa, ka a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ sɔb fɔsɔɔlaa kaar, ka a ŋmɛraa mɩ lɩɛb jɩ̃ɩ kaar jaa kpɩ̃n kpɩ̃n,
66006013	ka a ŋmɛrbie mɩ yi a saaju pɔrɔ loro a tẽe pɔ fɩka tɔ̃ɔ kara sɛsɛkpɛ̃ɛ na fu lɔb.
66006014	Be lɛ a saaju pilʋ̃ fɩka sɔ̃gãnãa ban pil, ka a tɔ̃n a jaa nɩ a dõdolsɩ a jaa mɩ ir a ba jiir.
66006015	Ka a tẽe nyã nãmɩne, a tẽe nyã nɩbɛrɛ, a fɔ̃ɔ dẽme, taraa dẽme, a gãdaar, nɩ a gbãgbaar ba jaa, nɩ a sumɩne ba jaa pãa sɔɔlɔ a tɔ̃n bɔɔr pɔ nɩ a tɔ̃n kʋsɩbɛ pɔ.
66006016	Ba pãa bʋɔlɔ na a tɔ̃n naa kʋsɩpãnsɩ, "Yɩ lo pii sɩ ka sɩ taa lɛ nyɛ a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju ɛ, na sɩ ta mɩ lɛ nyɛ a Pɛraabile suur ɛ!
66006017	A ba sukpɛ̃ɛ bɩbir vɩɛ naa, an lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ ara a ba niem?"
66007001	A anyã puor, n nyɛn a malakasɩ anaar ka ba ara a tẽe lõbobo anaar, na ba nyɔɔ a sɛsɛbɛ taa lɛ ɩka wʋ taa furo a wɛr pɔ, naa man pɔ, bɩɩ tɩɛ ju ɛ.
66007002	Be lɛ n nyɛ a malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ ka wʋ yi a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie waara na wʋ tara a Nãaŋmɩn vʋr sʋɔ jɩ̃nɛ. Wʋ bʋɔl naa a malakasɩ anaar bala nɩ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ ban kʋ sɔr ɩka ba sɔ̃ɔ a tẽe wʋ jaa naa man 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ ba,
66007003	"Yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a tẽe, naa man, naa tɩɩr ɛ, a sɩ 'yɔ̃ɔ a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ a ba gbersɩ pɔ baar."
66007004	N pãa wõ naa a nɩbɛ bala ban 'yɔ̃ɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ nɛɛ ka ba ɩ, nɩbɛ turo kɔbaa lɩjaayi nɩ anaar (144,000) na yi a Isɩral balbʋrsɩ pɔ.
66007005	A bala na yi a Juda bʋrɔ pɔ ban 'yɔ̃ɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ ɩn nɩbɛ turo pie naa yi (12,000), ka a Wuruben bʋrɔ mɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000), ka a Gad bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000),
66007006	ka a Aserɩ bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000), ka a Naftalɩ bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000), ka a Manasɛ bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000),
66007007	ka a Simeon bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000), ka a Levi bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000), ka a Isakar bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000),
66007008	ka a Jebulun bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000), ka a Josefʋ bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000), ka a Benjamin bʋrɔ mɩ ɩ a nɩbɛ turo pie nɩ ayi (12,000).
66007009	A anyã puor, n lɛ nyɛn nɩyɔɔ nɩrɛ na kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ba sɔr ɛ, ka ba yi a paalsɩ a jaa pɔ, balbʋrsɩ, nɩbʋrsɩ, 'yɛrbʋrsɩ a jaa pɔ, na ba ara a nãa dakɔɔ nɩ a Pɛraabile niem. Ba sun fɔpɩɛl tɩ tara bɛ wilsɩ a ba nuur pɔ.
66007010	Bala lɛ chɩlɛ 'yɛrɛ, "A faafʋ yi naa a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju nɩ a Pɛraabile sɛ̃."
66007011	Ka a malakasɩ bala na ara jilʋ̃ a nãa dakɔɔ, nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ, nɩ a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala gãn kpa a nãa dakɔɔ niem puoro a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛrɛ,
66007012	"A ɩ a lɛ! Nãaŋmɩn son pɛɛfʋ nɩ tɩɩr, nɩ yɛ̃, nɩ dãnfʋ, nɩ 'yɔ̃ɔfʋ, nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ fɔ̃ɔ. A ɩ a lɛ!"
66007013	Be lɛ a nɩkpɛ̃ɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ sʋʋr ma, "A bala na su a bʋ̃pɩɛl, ba boo lɛ, nɩ nyɩnɛ lɛ ba yi?"
66007014	Ka n 'yɛr ɩka, "Nɩkpɛ̃ɛ, fʋ̃ʋ ba lɛ bɔ̃ɔ ba." Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "A banyãna, bala lɛ yi a dɔɔyɛ kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ pɔ. Ba pɛɛn a ba fɔɔr nɩ a Pɛraabile jɩ̃ɩ.
66007015	Ala lɛ so ka ba ara a Nãaŋmɩn nãa dakɔɔ par tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ wʋ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ a wʋ puorfʋ yir. A 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju na 'yɩɛr pɔɔ ba.
66007016	Kɔ̃ kʋ̃ lɛ kpɛ ba go ɛ, kɔ̃nyũur mɩ kʋ̃ lɛ kpɛ ba go ɛ. Mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ kʋ̃ lɛ ŋme ba go ɛ, tʋl kʋ̃ lɛ kʋrɔ go ɛ.
66007017	A Pɛraabile na ara a nãa dakɔɔ sãlsɔɔ lɛ na chɩ̃nɛ ba. Wʋn ma ŋmaa ban chiin a nyɛvʋr kʋ̃ɔ par, ka Nãaŋmɩn pãa 'yɩɛr a ba nɩbikʋ̃ɔ a jaa bar."
66008001	Be lɛ a Pɛraabile 'lɔɔ a jɩ̃nsɩ ayopõi sʋɔ ka a saaju wʋ jaa ŋmaa vʋʋr jaa chɩr chɩr chɩr kor bɩ̃lãa.
66008002	Ka n nyɛ a malakasɩ ayopõi bala na ara a Nãaŋmɩn niem ka ba kʋ ba ɩɩl pɛɛlsɩ ayopõi.
66008003	A malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ na tara a sɛlma lapʋr, wa ara naa a bɔɔrlo bomo chʋmfʋ jie. Ba den a tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla ala kʋ wʋ ɩka wʋ de pʋɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ba jaa sʋɔrfʋsɩ a sɛlma bɔɔrlo bomo chʋmfʋ jie kʋ a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju.
66008004	A tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla jʋʋr yire naa a sɛlma lapʋr 'matãan a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ sʋɔrfʋ yi a malaka nũu pɔ, duoro a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃.
66008005	Be lɛ a malaka lɛ mʋ̃ɔ bũu bie a sɛlma bɔɔrlo bomo chʋmfʋ jie sɛɛ a lapʋr na wʋ lɔb bar ka a wɛr pɔ ka tãnfʋ, nɩ gɔ̃mɔ̃, nɩ saa nyɩɩrfʋ ka a tẽe wʋ jaa dam.
66008006	Ka a malakasɩ ayopõi bala na tara a ɩlɛ, go a pɛɛlfʋ.
66008007	A malaka 'lɔ na de nie pɛɛl naa a wʋ ɩɩl, ka a sakpʋlõbie nɩ bũu na 'matãan jɩ̃ɩ loro a wɛr pɔ. Ka a tẽe jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen di wʋ jaa, ka a tɩɩr mɩ jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen mɩ di lɔ̃ɔn a mɔ'yɔlɔ a jaa.
66008008	Ka a malakasɩ ayi sʋɔ mɩ pɛɛl a wʋ ɩɩl, ka ba 'lɔb bon na nyɛtãan tɔ̃kpɛ̃ɛ na nyɔɔ bũu 'yɔ̃ɔ a man pɔ. A man jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen lɩɛb jɩ̃ɩ,
66008009	ka a bʋ̃nɩbie mɩ jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen kpi, ka a gborbɛrɛ ala mɩ jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen mɩ wɛ.
66008010	Ka a malakasɩ ata sʋɔ mɩ pɛɛl a wʋ ɩɩl, ka a ŋmɛrbir kpɛ̃ɛ na 'lɩrɛ fɩka bũu yi a saaju lo a põnsɩ nɩ a bulsɩ jiir ata a jibʋ̃'yen pɔ.
66008011	A ŋmɛrbir yuor din, Bʋ̃tuo. Ka a kɔ̃n jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen be tuo, ka a nɩbɛ bala na nyũ a kɔ̃tuo ala, ka yɔɔ jie kpi.
66008012	A malakasɩ anaar sʋɔ pɛɛl naa a wʋ ɩɩl, ka ba ŋme a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen nɩ a ŋmɛraa jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen naa ŋmɛrbie ka ba jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen ɩ libe. A bɩbir jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen ba tara chãa ɛ, ka a ŋmɛraa naa ŋmɛrbie mɩ ba chaar a tɩ̃sɔɔ jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen ɛ.
66008013	Be lɛ n kaa naa wõ tuu na ɔɔrɔ be a saaju 'yɛrɛ nɩ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ, "Nɛbier! Nɛbier! Nɛbier! Yele na wa naa nɩsaal jaa na be a wɛr pɔ, ala ɩ a malakasɩ ata bala na chɛ wa pɛɛl naa a ba ɩlɛ."
66009001	A malakasɩ anũu sʋɔ na wa pɛɛl a wʋ ɩɩl, ka n nyɛ a ŋmɛrbir 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ yi a saaju lo a tẽe. A ŋmɛrbir nyã lɛ ba de a bɔɔ fulom pãn bir kʋ.
66009002	Wʋn wa yuo a bɔɔ fulom nyã nɛɛ, ka jʋʋr yire fɩka bũu kpɛ̃ɛ jʋʋr. A jʋʋr anyãna na yire a bɔɔ fulom nyãna pɔ liin pɔɔ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ naa tẽe wʋ jaa.
66009003	A jʋʋr anyãna pɔ lɛ soor yi yaar a tẽe wʋ jaa ka ba kʋ ba lɔɔ fɩka lɔ̃n lɔɔ.
66009004	Ba 'yɛr kʋ ba ɩka ba taa ɩrɛ wa ɔɔrɔ mɔɩ bɩɩ bʋ̃bul nɩ a tɩɛ vaar ɛ, tɩchɛ a dʋ̃nɔ̃ a nɩbɛ bala tɛɛ na ba tara a Nãaŋmɩn jɩ̃nɛ a ba gbersɩ pɔ ɛ.
66009005	Baa kʋ ba sɔr ɩka ba kʋrɔ ɛ, tɩchɛ ba ge a nɩbɛ ŋmɛrsɩ anũu. Ka a ba dʋ̃fʋ ɔɔr kaara fɩka lɔ̃ɔ na dʋ̃ nɩrɛ ɔɔrɔ.
66009006	A ber anyãna pɔ nɩbɛ na bʋɔrɔ na kũu tɩchɛ ba kʋ̃ nyɛ wʋ ɛ. Ban bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka ba kpi tɩchɛ a kũu kʋ̃ lɛ kʋ ba gba ɛ.
66009007	A soor nyɛtãan wiisɩ ban pɩ̃ɛ jɛɛr 'yɔ̃ɔ, ka a jur kaara fɩka sɛlma jupile ban su, ka a ba nin nyɛtãan nɩsaal nie.
66009008	A ba kɔɔl kaara fɩka pɔbɔ jukɔɔl, ka a nyɩmɛ mɩ kaara fɩka jukpɛ̃ɛ nyɩmɛ.
66009009	Ba tara na nyãa pɔɔrsɩ ka a kaara fɩka kue, ka a pɩbɛ dɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ fɩka torkosɩ a wiisɩ na tɔɔrɔ joro chiine jɛɛr jie.
66009010	Ba tara na jʋɛ dʋ̃nɔ̃ nɩ lɔ̃n kaar, a jʋɛ ala tara na fɔ̃ɔ na dʋ̃n nɩbɛ ge ba ŋmɛrsɩ anũu.
66009011	Ba tara na nãa na kaara ba, 'lɔ lɛ a malaka 'lɔ na kaara a bɔɔ fulom 'lɔ. Heburu nɩbɛ bʋɔlɔ wʋ naa, Abadɔn, ka a Greek nɩbɛ mɩ bʋɔlɔ, Apolyɔn. A par lɛ, sɔ̃sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃.
66009012	A nɛbier 'lɔ na de nie lɛ a nyã na tal, tɩchɛ ka a ayi sʋɔ chɛnɛ be puor waara.
66009013	Ka a malakasɩ ayʋɔb sʋɔ pɛɛl a wʋ ɩɩl, n wõn kɔkɔr na yire a sɛlma tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla chʋmfʋ jie kpʋ̃kpʋɛ, be lɛ ba ma chʋm a kãnyũu na be a Nãaŋmɩn niem.
66009014	A kɔkɔr 'yɛr kʋ a malaka ayʋɔb sʋɔ 'lɔ na tara a ɩɩl, "For a malakasɩ anaar bala ban lũ a be a Yufɩrɩtɩ põn kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ."
66009015	A wʋ for a malakasɩ anaar ba nyãna ban dɔ̃ɔ lũ gun a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃, a bɩbir 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ nɩ a chuu 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ naa yuon 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ ɩka ba kʋ a nɩsaal jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen bar.
66009016	Ka a bala na do a wiisɩ ba bʋɔl naa a ba nɛɛ fʋn kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ba sɔr ɛ.
66009017	A wiisɩ nɩ a bala na do ɩn nyɛ a jãna pɔ, a nyãa pɔɔrsɩ mʋ̃ɔ naa fɩka bũu, ka amɩne mɩ ɩ bufulo, ka amɩne mɩ ɩ bʋ̃dʋɔr. Ka a wiisɩ jur nyɛtãan jubɛrɛ jur, ka a bũu jʋʋr nɩ jerbɩ mɩ yire a ba nɛɛ pɔ.
66009018	A gefʋ ata ala na yi a wiisɩ nɛɛ pɔ lɛ, bũu, nɩ jʋʋr, nɩ jerbɩ, ala lɛ ba kʋn nɩbɛ jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen.
66009019	A wiisɩ anyã fɔ̃ɔ be naa a ba nɛɛ pɔ naa jʋɛ pɔ, a ba jʋɛ kaara fɩka waba naa tara jur, ala lɛ ba de gere nɩ a nɩsaal.
66009020	A nɩsaalba bala na chɛ, na baa kpin a gefʋ nyã ɛ, ba sɔɔ bar a tɩbɛ ala ban maal nɩ a ba nuur ɛ. Ba chɛnɛ na puoro a sɩdɛbɛ, nɩ a bʋtɩbɛ ban maal a sɛlma, nɩ a kur pɩɛl, nɩ a kur jɩɛ, nɩ a kusɩbɛ, nɩ a daar na ba wõnõ 'yɛr ɛ, ba kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ chen ɛ.
66009021	Baa mɩ lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr bar a nɩkʋyelsɩ, nɩ sɔyelsɩ, nɩ sɛ̃sɛ̃yelsɩ, nɩ nãnyiyelsɩ ɛ.
66010001	N lɛ nyɛn a malaka kpɛ̃ɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ na yi a saaju suro waara. Wʋ vaar naa julõjuur ka a sagõgoraa dɔɔl a jum. A nie kaara fɩka mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ, ka a gbɛɛ mɩ kaara fɩka bũu lɩraa.
66010002	Wʋ tara na gãn bile na yuo a wʋ nũu pɔ, na wʋ de a nũsʋ̃ɔ gbɛr 'lɔr a man pɔ tɩ a gʋbaa gbɛr dɔɔl a gogoro ju,
66010003	tɩ na wʋ pãa tãn kpɛ̃ɔ jaa fɩka jukpɛ̃ɛ na uor. Wʋn wa tãn a lɛ ka a kɔkɔɛ ɩ ayopõi mɩ tãn satanaa kaar.
66010004	An wa tãn a gbɛɛ ayopõi a lɛ, ka n ta bʋɔrɔ ɩka n sɛb tɩchɛ n wõn kɔkɔr na yi a saaju 'yɛr, "A tãnfʋ ayopõi ala na 'yɛr sɔɔl bar, ta sɛb bin ɛ."
66010005	Be lɛ a malaka 'lɔ ɩn nyɛ na 'lɔr a nũsʋ̃ɔ gbɛr a man pɔ tɩ dɔɔl a a gʋba gbɛr a gogoro ju, jɛɛn a nũsʋ̃ɔ a saaju.
66010006	Wʋ pɔn naa a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na be be jaa kpo kpo, 'lɔ lɛ mɛ a saaju, nɩ a tẽe, nɩ a man, nɩ bomo a jaa na be a ba pɔ, "A kʋ̃ lɛ kor go ɛ!
66010007	Tɩchɛ a bɩbir 'lɔ a malakasɩ ayopõi sʋɔ na wa pɛɛl a wʋ ɩɩl, a Nãaŋmɩn yelsɔɔlaa na pãa maal baar nɩtãa a lɛ wʋn man kʋ a wʋ gbãgbaar 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ."
66010008	Be lɛ a kɔkɔr 'lɔ ɩn dɔ̃ɔ wõ a saaju lɛ 'yɛr kʋ ma go, "Chen tɩ de a gãn bile 'lɔ na yuo a malaka 'lɔ na ara a man pɔ naa gogoro ju nũu pɔ."
66010009	Ka n chen a malaka sɛ̃ tɩ sʋɔr wʋ ɩka wʋ kʋ ma a gãn bile. Ka wʋ 'yɛr, "De 'wɔb, wʋn mire naa a fʋ pʋɔ pɔ tɩ nʋ̃mɔ̃ a fʋ nɛɛ pɔ sɩkãa kaar."
66010010	N den a gãn bile a malaka nũu pɔ 'wɔb. Ka wʋ nʋ̃mɔ̃ a n nɛɛ pɔ a sɩkãa kaar, tɩchɛ ɩn wa vɔl baar, ka wʋ mire a pʋɔ pɔ.
66010011	A ba lɛ 'yɛr kʋ ma go, "'Yɛr 'yɛr kʋ a nɩbʋrɔ, nɩ paalsɩ, nɩ 'yɛrbʋrsɩ nɩ a nãmɩne."
66011001	Be lɛ a nɩrɛ kɔ̃ɔ de dãgbal na kaara a damanaa kaar kʋ ma tɩ 'yɛr, "Chen tɩ man a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir nɩ a bɔɔr lofʋ jie na fʋ sɔr a nɩbɛ bala na puoro a be.
66011002	Tɩchɛ taa ɩrɛ wa mana a yõo ɛ, bojũu be lɛ a bala na ba ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ ɛ, na be 'mu 'mulo a tẽchɛchɛ nyãna ŋmɛrsɩ lɩjaayi nɩ ayi.
66011003	Ɩ̃n kʋ naa a n yelmɩ̃ɛ dãasɩɛ nɩbɛ ayi ka ba su fɔjãrsɩ tɩ mʋɔlɔ na ba 'yɛrɛ ber tur dɔɔl kɔɔr ayi nɩ lɩjaata (1,260)."
66011004	A dãasɩɛ dẽme ayi bala ɩ naa a kãa tɩɩr ayi nɩ a fɩ̃tɩnɛ dɔɔlfʋ jie jiir ayi, ba ara naa a Soro nyã na ɩ a wɛr wʋ jaa niem.
66011005	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ bʋɔrɔ naa ɩka wʋ maal ba bier, bũu ma yi naa a ba nɛɛ pɔ di a bala na ɩ a ba dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃sɩ. Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tɩɛr a ba sɔ̃ɔfʋ ma kpi.
66011006	A nɩbɛ bala tara na kpɛ̃ɔ na nyɔɔ saa a saaju ka a saa kʋ̃ wa a sɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban mʋɔlɔ ɛ. Ba mɩ tara na kpɛ̃ɔ na lɩɛb a kɔ̃n a jaa ka a ɩ jɩ̃ɩ, na ba mɩ na tʋ̃ɔ vɛ̃ ka yelbier wa a tẽe pɔ sɔ̃ɔ jaa ban bʋɔrɔ.
66011007	Ala ɩ ba wa baar naa a dãasɩɛ difʋ, a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ na yi a bɔɔ fulom 'lɔ pɔ na ŋmaan ban jɛɛr na wʋ tʋ̃ɔ ba na wʋ kʋ.
66011008	Ka a ba ɩ̃gãma gã be a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ sɔkpɛ̃ɛ ju. A tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã lɛ ba lɔɔrɔ sʋkpa bʋɔlɔ nɩ Sodom bɩɩ Ijipitɩ, be lɛ ba kpa a ba Soro a daa ju.
66011009	Nɩbʋrɔ, nɩ 'yɛrbʋrɔ, nɩ balsɩ ba jaa, nɩ paalsɩ a jaa na kaara naa a ba ɩ̃gãma ban tɔr a ũufʋ bɩbie ata nɩ bʋ̃ŋmaa.
66011010	Nʋ̃ɔ na kpɛ̃n a nɩbɛ na kpɩɛrɛ a wɛr pɔ ka ba chɩlɛ kʋrɔ taa bonsɩ, bojũu ba kʋ naa a 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ayi banyãna na dɔ̃ɔ ge a wɛr nɩbɛ.
66011011	Tɩchɛ a bɩbie ata nɩ a bʋ̃ŋmaa ala na wa po, Nãaŋmɩn 'yɔ̃ɔ ban nyɛvʋr ka ba lɛ ir ɩ vʋɛ, ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a bala na nyɛ ba.
66011012	A 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ ayi banyãna pãa wõn nɛkpɛ̃ɛ na yi saaju 'yɛr, "Yɩ do wa ka." Ka ba tu a julõjuur pɔ duoro a saaju ka a ba dɔ̃dɔ̃mɔ̃sɩ kaara ba.
66011013	Be lɛ ajienaa ka a tẽe mii ka a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ yie jiir pie jibʋ̃'yen lo naa kʋ nɩbɛ tur ayopõi (7,000) ka a dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ a bala na chɛ a ba pɛɛrɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na be a saaju.
66011014	A nɛbier ayi sʋɔ lɛ a nyã na po, tɩchɛ a ata sʋɔ mɩ turo naa.
66011015	A malakasɩ ayopõi sʋɔ pɛɛl naa a wʋ ɩɩl, ka a kɔkɔyɔɔ 'yɛrɛ be a saaju, "A wɛr nyã nãalʋ̃ʋ ɩ naa a sɩ Soro nɩ a wʋ Nɩ-iraa nãalʋ̃ʋ, 'lɔ lɛ na di a nãa jaa kpo kpo."
66011016	A nɩbɛrɛ lɩjɛr nɩ anaar bala na jɩ̃nɛ a ba nãa dakɔɔr ju a Nãaŋmɩn niem gãn kpa tẽe puor a Nãaŋmɩn
66011017	tɩ 'yɛrɛ, "Sɩ puor naa a Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ, 'Lɔ lɛ ɩ, nɩ 'Lɔ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be, bojũu wʋ den a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ piel kaara nɩ a wɛr wʋ jaa.
66011018	A paalsɩ vʋ̃n fʋn nɛɛ ka fʋ suur mɩ dire. A sɔ̃ɔ ta naa ka fʋn tɔɔr a kũn 'yɛr, na fʋn yab a fʋ gbãgbaar na ɩ a 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ lɔ̃ɔn a fʋ nɩbɛ naa bala na 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a fʋ yuor, a bil naa bɛrɛ ba jaa, na fʋn sɔ̃ɔ a bala na sɔ̃ɔ a wɛr."
66011019	Ka a Nãaŋmɩn yir na be a saaju pãn pãa yuo ka ba nyɛ a nɛtɩraa daka be a yir pɔ. Ka saa nyɩɩrfʋ, gɔ̃mɔ̃, nɩ tãnfʋ, ka a tẽe wʋ jaa mii, ka a sakpʋlõbibɛrɛ loro.
66012001	A nɛ'maa yelbɛrɛ na yi a saaju ka a pɔɔ vaar mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ fɩka fɔbaa tɩ dɔɔl a gbɛɛ a ŋmɛraa ju, ka a ŋmɛrbie pie nɩ ayi ɩ nãa jupil ka wʋ su.
66012002	Pʋɔ lɛ wʋ tara ka wʋ dɔɔfʋ ta ka wʋ kõnõ nɩ.
66012003	Be lɛ ka a nɛ'maa yele ɩ̃sʋɔ lɛ yi a saaju kaara fɩka dajɩl na ɩ jɩɛ na wʋ tara jur ayopõi nɩ ɩlɛ pie ka a nãa jupile be a jur pɔ.
66012004	A wʋ jʋʋr pɩɩr naa a ŋmɛrbie jiir ata jibʋ̃'yen a saaju 'lɔb a tẽe. Tɩ ara gu a pɔɔ 'lɔ na bʋɔrɔ a dɔɔfʋ ɩka 'lɔ wa dɔɔ wʋ vɔl a bie.
66012005	A pɔɔ dɔɔn a bie ka wʋ ɩ dabile, 'lɔ lɛ na kaara a paalsɩ a jaa nɩ la kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ na kaara a kur dãgbal kaar. Ba jãan a pɔɔ bie nyã don a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ ka wʋ tɩ be a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ pɔ.
66012006	Tɩ ka a pɔɔ mɩ jo kpɛ a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ na wʋ tɩ be a jie Nãaŋmɩn na chɔɔr bar ka ban kaara wʋ maal ber tur kɔɔr ayi dɔɔl lɩjaata (1,260).
66012007	Ka a jɛɛr lo be a saaju. Maɩkɩl nɩ a malakasɩ jɛɛr nɩ naa a dajɩl, ka a dajɩl nɩ a wʋ malakasɩ mɩ lɩɛb jɛɛrɛ nɩ a Maɩkɩl nɩ a wʋ malakasɩ.
66012008	Tɩchɛ ba tʋ̃ɔ naa a dajɩl nɩ a wʋ malakasɩ, dii ba bar a be a saaju.
66012009	Ba lɔb a dajɩl kpɛ̃ɛ nyã bar a yõo, a kõr waa 'lɔ̃nɔ̃ na ɩ a dɛɛr sʋɔ, nɩ a Satan, 'lɔ lɛ bɛlʋ̃ a wɛr nɩbɛ ba jaa. Ba lɔb wʋn bar ka a wɛr pɔ, nɩ a wʋ malakasɩ.
66012010	Be lɛ n wõ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ na 'yɛr be a saaju, "Pʋ̃pãanyã, a faafʋ bɩbir vɩɛ naa, a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn wiil naa a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ, nɩ a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ, nɩ a wʋ Nɩ-iraa kpɛ̃ɔ. Bojũu a 'lɔ na bɛrɛ a sɩ yɛɛr nɛɛ, 'lɔ lɛ bɛrɛ ba a nɛɛ a Nãaŋmɩn niem mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ, ba daa wʋn lɔb.
66012011	Ba tʋ̃ɔ wʋ naa nɩ a Pɛraabile jɩ̃ɩ nɩ a ba dãasɩɛ 'yɛrbie. Ba sɔɔn kũu na baa de a ba nyɛvʋr ka wʋ ɩ bon ɛ.
66012012	A lɛ jũu, saaju naa bala na kpɩɛrɛ a be, yɩ chɩlɛ! Tɩchɛ nɛbier ben a yɩn na be a wɛr nɩ a man pɔ, yɩn din dɔɔyɛ, bojũu a dɛɛr sʋɔ suun a yɩ sɛ̃! Ka a wʋ suur dire, bojũu a wʋ ber ba waa ɛ."
66012013	Lɛ a dajɩl na wa nyɛ ka a ɩ tẽe lɛ wʋ lo, wʋ dire naa a pɔɔ 'lɔ na dɔɔ a dabile.
66012014	Ka ba kʋ a pɔɔ tuu kpɛ̃ɛ pibɛ ayi, ɩka wʋ ɔɔ chen a jie ban chɔɔr bar be a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ, be lɛ ban tɩ kaara wʋ yuom ata nɩ bʋ̃ŋmaa ka a waa taa pɔɔ wʋ ɛ.
66012015	Be lɛ ka a waa chɩr kʋ̃ɔ a nɛɛ pɔ põn kʋ̃ɔ kaar, ɩka a di a pɔɔ,
66012016	tɩchɛ ka a tẽe sʋ̃ʋ a pɔɔ haa a nɛɛ nyũ a kʋ̃ɔ ala a dajɩl na chɩr a nɛɛ pɔ.
66012017	Ka a dajɩl pãa nyɛ suur 'yɔ̃ɔ a pɔɔ na wʋ chen tɩ ŋmaan a pɔɔ bibiir bala na chɛ jɛɛr. A bala na turo a Nãaŋmɩn nɛɛ na ba mɩ tara a Yesu 'yɛr yelmɩ̃ɛ.
66013001	Ka a dajɩl ara a man gogoro nɛɛ. N nyɛn mɔdʋ̃ɔ na yire a man pɔ na wʋ tara jur ayopõi tɩ bul ɩlɛ pie ka a nãa jupile su a ɩlɛ ala pɔ. A jur ala pɔ yoe ben be na fere sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ Nãaŋmɩn yuor.
66013002	A mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn nyɛ nyɛntãan gbɔ̃gbɔ̃ɔ tɩchɛ ka a gbɛɛ kaara fɩka pɛɛlaa gbɛɛ ka a nɛɛ mɩ kaara fɩka jukpɛ̃ɛ nɛɛ. Ka a dajɩl de a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ a wʋ nãa dakɔɔ nɩ a wʋ tʋ̃ɔfʋ kʋ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ̃nɔ̃.
66013003	A mɔdʋ̃ɔ ju ɩ̃sʋɔ kaara fɩka bon ban chɛ ɩrɛ na kʋ tɩchɛ ka a chɛfʋ jie 'lɔ 'mɔ̃ pɔɔ. Nɛɛ 'maan a nɩrɛ jaa na be a wɛr pɔ tɩ na ba turo a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ.
66013004	Ka nɩrɛ jaa pãa pɛɛrɛ a dajɩl bojũu 'lɔ lɛ de a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ na ba mɩ pɛɛrɛ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ 'yɛrɛ nɩ tɩ sʋrɔ, "An lɛ kaara a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nyã kaar? Nɩ an lɛ na tʋ̃ɔ ŋmaan wʋ jɛɛr?"
66013005	A mɔdʋ̃ɔ nyã tara na nɛɛ na 'yɛrɛ ɛ jɩ̃jɩɩr 'yɛr na wʋ fere, wʋ tara na sɔr ɩka wʋ 'yɛr a wʋ yobɔ 'yɛr maal ŋmɛrsɩ lɩjaayi nɩ ayi (42).
66013006	A wʋ 'yɛrbie chɩrɛ nɩ naa Nãaŋmɩn na wʋ fere sɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn yuor nɩ a jie 'lɔ wʋn be nɩ a bala na kpɩɛrɛ a saaju.
66013007	Ba kʋ wʋn sɔr ɩka wʋ jɛb a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ na wʋ tʋ̃ɔ ba na wʋ mɩ tʋ̃ɔ a nɩbʋrɔ, nɩ 'yɛrbʋrɔ, nɩ balbʋrɔ, nɩ paalsɩ.
66013008	A bala ba jaa yuor na ba dɔ̃ɔ sɛb a Pɛraabile ban dɔ̃ɔ kʋ a nyɛvʋr gãn pɔ ɛ, tɩ a wɛr wa mɛ, na gbur dumo puor a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nyãna.
66013009	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ na tara toor, wʋ chɛlɛ.
66013010	Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa nyɔɔfʋ lɛ ban nyɔɔ wʋ, ban nyɔɔ wʋn chiin. Ala ɩ sɔkpɛ̃ɛ mɩ lɛ ban kʋn ɩ̃sʋɔ, a sɔkpɛ̃ɛ lɛ ban kʋn wʋ. A lɛ jũu a bala na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ, ba tara kãnyir nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ.
66013011	N pãa lɛ nyɛn a mɔdʋ̃ɔ ɩ̃sʋɔ na yire a tẽe tara ɩlɛ ayi fɩka pɛraabile tɩ 'yɛrɛ fɩka a dajɩl.
66013012	Wʋ yin de a mɔdʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ kpɛ̃ɔ na wʋ wiil wʋ mɩ̃ɛ a mɔdʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ niem tɩ fɩr a nɩbɛ ba jaa na be ka a wɛr pɔ ka ba gbur dumo puor a mɔdʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ chɛfʋ jie na 'mɔ pɔɔ.
66013013	Wʋ tʋ̃n nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃sɩ na wʋ gba ma vɛ̃ ka bũu yi saaju suu wa a tẽe ka nɩbɛ ba jaa nyɛ.
66013014	A wʋ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ anyãna jũu, ba kʋ wʋn kpɛ̃ɔ ka wʋ de a mɔdʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ jie, na wʋ bɛl a wɛr nɩbɛ. Ka wʋ 'yɛr ba ka ba mɛ bʋtɩbɛ 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ nɩ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ ban dɔ̃ɔ chen a sʋɔ tɩ wʋ 'mɔ pɔɔ.
66013015	Ba kʋ wʋn sɔr ɩka wʋ kʋ a bʋtɩɩ 'lɔ nyɛvʋr wʋn mɛ ka wʋ nyɛtãan a mɔdʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ, ka wʋ na tʋ̃ɔ 'yɛr ka ba kʋ a bala na tɔr a bʋtɩɩ puorfʋ.
66013016	Wʋ mɩ fɩr nɩrɛ jaa, ka bile lɛ wʋ ɩ bɩɩ kpɛ̃ɛ lɛ, taraa sʋɔ bɩɩ nɔ̃ɔ sʋɔ, sumɩne bɩɩ gbãgbaa, ka ba 'yɔ̃ɔ ba jaa jɩ̃nsɩ a nũsʋ̃ɔ nũu pɔ bɩɩ a gberaa pɔ.
66013017	Nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ daara bɩɩ da bon ka baa 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ a jɩ̃nɛ na ɩ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ yuor bɩɩ a wʋ jɩ̃nɛ 'lɔ na ɩ a wʋ yuor ɛ.
66013018	Ka 'lɔ yɛ̃ 'yɛr lɛ, ala ɩ nɩrɛ tara na bɔ̃ɔfʋ, wʋn tʋ̃ɔ sɔr a mɔdʋ̃ɔ sɛbie an ɩ nɩsaal sɛbie lɛ. A sɛbie ɩ naa kɔɔr ayʋɔb dɔɔl lɩjaata nɩ ayʋɔb (666).
66014001	Be lɛ n kaa nyɛ a Pɛraabile ka wʋ 'mataa ara nɩ nɩbɛ turo kɔbaa lɩjaayi nɩ anaar (144,000) a Jiyon tɔ̃ɔ ju ka wʋ yuor nɩ a Sãa yuor sɛb 'mar a ba gbersɩ pɔ.
66014002	N wõn kɔkɔɛ a saaju na gɔ̃nɔ̃ fɩka kɔ̃kpɛ̃ɛ na joro bɩɩ saa na tãn. A gɔ̃mɔ̃ mɩ kaara fɩka kõrõjomsɩ ban ŋmiere.
66014003	Ba yiele naa yiel paalaa a nãa dakɔɔ niem nɩ a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala nɩ a nɩbɛrɛ bala niem. Nɩrɛ jaa ba be be na tʋ̃ɔ a yiel jãn ɛ, ka a nɩbɛ turo kɔbaa lɩjaayi nɩ anaar (144,000) bala tɛɛ a Nãaŋmɩn na faa ka a wɛr pɔ ba lɛ ɛ.
66014004	A banyãna lɛ ba sɔ̃ɔ ba mɩ̃ɛ nɩ pɔbɔ ɛ, bojũu ba gun ba mɩ̃ɛ ɩ chɛchɛ, na ba ma turo a Pɛraabile jie jaa wʋn chiine, bala lɛ ba da de kʋ Nãaŋmɩn fɩka bʋ̃dɔ̃ɔ ban de kʋ Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Pɛraabile.
66014005	Baa haa nɛɛ ŋmaa jir ɛ. Baa tara chɛfʋ bɩ̃lãa jaa ɛ.
66014006	N pãa lɛ nyɛn a malakasɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ na ɔɔrɔ be a saaju tɩ tara a 'yɛr kpo kpo bʋɔrɔ ɩka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ a bala na be ka a wɛr pɔ, nɩ paalsɩ a jaa, nɩ balbʋrsɩ a jaa, nɩ 'yɛrbʋrsɩ a jaa, nɩ nɩbʋrsɩ a jaa.
66014007	Wʋ tãn na nɩ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ, "Yɩ joro a Nãaŋmɩn dãbɩ̃ɛ na yɩ kʋrɔ wʋ tɩɩr, bojũu a wʋ bɩbir vɩɛ naa ka wʋn tɔɔr a nɩbɛ 'yɛr. Yɩ puor wʋ, 'lɔ lɛ maal a saaju, nɩ a wɛr, nɩ a man nɩ a kʋ̃ɔ yifʋ jiir."
66014008	A malakasɩ ayi sʋɔ mɩ tun wa 'yɛrɛ, "Wʋ wɛl naa, wʋ wɛl naa, a Babilon tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã 'lɔ lɛ maal a paalsɩ a jaa a ba nyũ a wʋ sɛ̃sɛ̃yele dãa ala na tɔɔ Nãaŋmɩn suur waan."
66014009	Ka a malakasɩ ata sʋɔ mɩ tu wa 'yɛrɛ nɩ kɔkɔkpɛ̃ɛ, "Ala wa ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa puor naa a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nyãna naa bʋtɩɩ nyãna ban mɛ a wʋ kaar, na wʋ sɔɔ ka ba 'yɔ̃ɔ wʋ a jɩ̃nɛ a gberaa pɔ bɩɩ a nũu pɔ,
66014010	wʋ mɩ na nyũn a dãa ala na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn suur, ala lɛ ba pʋr 'yɔ̃ɔ a ŋmele pɔ na ɩ a suur. Ban ge wʋ naa nɩ a jerbɩ bũu na dire a malaka chɛchɛsɩ bala naa Pɛraabile niem.
66014011	A ba gefʋ jʋʋr na uro ba tara ŋmaafʋ ɛ. Pɛ̃nfʋ ba be be kʋ a bala na gbur dumo puor a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nɩ a bʋtɩɩ 'lɔ ban mɛ a wʋ kaar mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ bɩɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ ɛ, bɩɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na sɔɔ de a jɩ̃nɛ na ɩ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ yuor ɛ."
66014012	A lɛ jũu, a bala na ɩ Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ na ba turo a wʋ nɛɛ na ba mɩ ara nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ kʋ a Yesu ba tara kãnyir.
66014013	N pãa lɛ wõn kɔkɔr na yi a saaju 'yɛrɛ, "Sɛb a anyãna an yi a dɩna chiine, pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ na kpi a Soro sɔr pɔ." "Ɔ̃ɔ," lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn Sɩɛ 'yɛr, "Ban pɛ̃n naa a ba dɔɔyɛ pɔ. Bojũu a lɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ tʋ̃, na turo ba naa."
66014014	N lɛ kãan nyɛ julõjupɩla, ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a julõjuur ju kaara fɩka nɩsaal bie na wʋ su sɛlma jupil a ju pɔ, tɩ na wʋ tara bʋ̃ŋma sɔkpɛ̃ɛ na dire a nũu pɔ.
66014015	Be lɛ a malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ yi be a Nãaŋmɩn yir wa bʋɔlɔ 'yɛrɛ kpɛ̃ɔ jaa kʋrɔ a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a julõjuur ju, "De a sɔkpɛ̃ɛ na fʋ piel tʋ̃mɔ̃ bojũu a tʋ̃mɔ̃ sɔ̃ɔ ta naa, bojũu a wɛr nyã ban na ŋma mʋ̃ɔ naa."
66014016	Lɛ lɛ a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a julõjuur ju jaal a sɔkpɛ̃ɛ bar a wɛr pɔ na wʋ ŋma a wɛr wʋ jaa.
66014017	A malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ na yi a be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir a saaju na wʋ mɩ tara a bʋ̃ŋma sɔkpɛ̃ɛ diir ɩ̃sʋɔ.
66014018	Ka a malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ mɩ 'lɔ lɛ kaara a bũu ka wʋ wa yi a be a tɩ̃ɩ nyũu vɩla chʋmfʋ jie bʋɔl a 'lɔ na tara a bʋ̃ŋma sɔkpɛ̃ɛ diir kpɛ̃ɔ jaa tɩ 'yɛr, "De a fʋ bʋ̃ŋma sɔkpɛ̃ɛ diir 'lɔ na fʋ ŋman a tɩɛ wɔ̃mɔ̃, a wɛr lɛ ɩ a tɩɛ ka wʋ wɔ̃mɔ̃ mʋ̃ɔ."
66014019	A malaka jaal a wʋ sɔkpɛ̃ɛ bar ka a wɛr pɔ ka wʋ ŋmara a wɔ̃mɔ̃ kpaara 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a be ban ma nɛɛrɛ ŋmɛrɛ, na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn suur.
66014020	Ba nɛɛrɛ ban a be a nɛŋmɛrfʋ jie a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ yõo, ka a jɩ̃ɩ joro a ŋmɛrfʋ jie ɩrɛ na ta mɛl kɔɔr ayi ka a wii mɩ ma kpɛ ka a nɛɛ 'lɔr.
66015001	N nyɛ naa a nɛ'maa yelwiilaa jɩ̃nɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ a saaju, malakasɩ ayopõi na tara wõmsɩ ayopõi, ala lɛ ɩ a baaraa na vɛ̃ ka Nãaŋmɩn suur lo.
66015002	N lɛ nyɛn bon na kaara fɩka man kʋ̃ɔ jaa wel wel nyɩlɛ chãana kaar lɔ̃ɔtãan bũu ka nɩbɛ ara a wʋ gogoro par. Bala lɛ jɛb tʋ̃ɔ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nɩ a wʋ bʋtɩɩ nɩ a yuor jɩ̃nɛ. Nãaŋmɩn kʋ ban kõrõjomsɩ
66015003	ka ba yiele nɩ a wʋ gbãgbaa Mosesɩ nɩ a Pɛraabile yiele 'yɛrɛ, "A Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ, a fʋ tʋ̃mɔ̃ 'maan nɛɛ tɩ põn bar, fʋ ɩn nɩtor nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a nãmɩne ba jaa Nãa.
66015004	An lɛ kʋ̃ joro a fʋ̃ʋ Soro dãbɩ̃ɛ na wʋ kʋ a fʋ yuor tɩɩr ɛ? Bojũu fʋ̃ʋ tɛɛ lɛ ɩ chɛchɛ. A paalsɩ a jaa na wa gãn kpa tẽe a fʋ niem, bojũu nɩrɛ jaa nyɛ naa a fʋ tʋ̃torsɩ."
66015005	Bojũu a anyã puor, n kãan nyɛ a saaju ka a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir a jichɛchɛ 'lɔ na ɩ a dãasɩɛ jie ka wʋ yuo.
66015006	Ka a malakasɩ ayopõi yi a jichɛchɛ nyãna na ba tara a Nãaŋmɩn suur wõmsɩ ayopõi sun bʋ̃pɩɛl na nyɩlɛ ka a sɛlma bʋ̃lunsɩ bãbɩ̃ a ba nyãn pɔ.
66015007	Be lɛ ka a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala ɩ̃sʋɔ kʋ a malakasɩ ayopõi bala sɛlma laar ayopõi na sɛɛr nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na be be jaa kpo kpo suur.
66015008	Ka a jʋʋr sɛɛ a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir yi a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr nɩ a wʋ kpɛ̃ɔ pɔ, ka nɩrɛ jaa kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ kpɛ a puorfʋ yir ka a malakasɩ ba wa baar a Nãaŋmɩn suur wõmsɩ ala baar ɛ.
66016001	N wõn nɛkpɛ̃ɛ na yi a be a puorfʋ yir 'yɛrɛ kʋrɔ a malakasɩ ayopõi bala, "Yɩ chen tɩ kpaar a Nãaŋmɩn suur a laar pɔ bar a wɛr."
66016002	Ka a malaka dɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ chen tɩ kpaar a wʋ laa bar ka a tẽe ka a natɩdɛbɛ na bɩɛrɛ tɛ a nɩbɛ bala na tara a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ jɩ̃nɛ tɩ mɩ gbur dumo puor a bʋtɩɩ.
66016003	A malaka ayi sʋɔ mɩ kpaar a wʋ laa bar a man pɔ, ka a kʋ̃ɔ lɩɛb fɩka kũu jɩ̃ɩ, ka a bʋ̃vʋʋrsɩ a jaa na be a man pɔ kpi.
66016004	A malaka ata sʋɔ mɩ kpaar a wʋ laa 'yɔ̃ɔ a põnsɩ nɩ kʋlsɩ pɔ, ka a kɔ̃n mɩ lɩɛb jɩ̃ɩ.
66016005	Be lɛ n wõ a malaka 'lɔ na kaara a kɔ̃n 'yɛr, "Fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ a Torfʋ Sʋɔ, a fʋ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ nyã tor naa, fʋ̃ʋ lɛ ɩ, fʋ̃ʋ mɩ lɛ dɔ̃ɔ be be Chɛchɛ Sʋɔ a yelsɩ anyãna fʋn tɔɔr a 'yɛr jũu.
66016006	Bojũu a putudẽme bala lɛ kʋ a fʋ nɩbɛ nɩ a fʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ a fʋ kʋ ba a jɩ̃ɩ ɩka ba nyũ, a lɛ sɛɛn ba naa."
66016007	Be lɛ n wõ kɔkɔr na 'yɛr be a bɔɔr lofʋ jie, "Ɔ̃ɔ, n Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ, a fʋ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ tɩ mɩ tor."
66016008	A malakasɩ anaar sʋɔ kpaar a wʋ laa 'yɔ̃ɔ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ ka wʋ tara kpɛ̃ɔ vuul a nɩbɛ nɩ bũu.
66016009	A mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ tʋl vuul ba naa tɩ ba chɛnɛ tʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn yuor an ɩ 'lɔ lɛ tara a gefʋ anyãna a jaa kpɛ̃ɔ na baa lɩɛb ba tɩɛr kʋ wʋ tɩɩr ɛ.
66016010	A malakasɩ anũu sʋɔ kpaar a wʋ laa 'yɔ̃ɔ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nãa dakɔɔ ju, ka a wʋ nãalʋ̃ʋ wʋ jaa lɩɛb libe, ka a wõnõ a nɩbɛ ka ba ɔɔrɔ jãlbie
66016011	tɩ chɛnɛ tʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn nyã na be a saaju a ba natɩɛ nɩ an bɩɛrɛ ba jũu. Tɩchɛ baa lɩɛb a ba tɩɛr bar a ba tʋ̃dɛbɛ ɛ.
66016012	A malakasɩ ayʋɔb sʋɔ mɩ kpaar naa a wʋ laa 'yɔ̃ɔ a Yufɩrɩtɩ põn kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ, ka a kʋ̃ɔ sɩr chɔɔr a sɔr bar kʋ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie nãmɩne.
66016013	N lɛ nyɛn a sɩdɛbɛ na kaara pãtɩɛ kaar ka a yire a bon 'lɔ na kaara a dajɩl kaar nɛɛ pɔ, naa lɛ yire a mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ mɩ nɛɛ pɔ, naa mɩ lɛ yire a jir ŋmarba 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ nɛɛr pɔ.
66016014	A sɩɩr anyã ɩ naa a tɩɩ sɩɩr na tʋ̃nɔ̃ nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃sɩ. Ba chen naa a wɛr wʋ jaa nãmɩne sɛ̃ tɩ lɔ̃ɔ taa na ŋmaan a Nãaŋmɩn Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ jɛɛr a wʋ bɩbir kpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ daar.
66016015	"Nyɛ ɩn wan nãnyie kaar. Bɔɔsʋ̃n sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ na ba gur ɛ, tɩ mɩ tara a wʋ bʋ̃sursɩ jɛn na wʋ kʋ̃ wa chiine nɩ sal'mʋɔr ka a ɩrɛ wʋ vĩ ɛ."
66016016	Be lɛ a sɩɩr lɔ̃ɔtaa a nãmɩne a jie 'lɔ a Heburu nɩbɛ na bʋɔlɔ Amagedɔn.
66016017	A malakasɩ ayopõi sʋɔ kpaar naa a wʋ laa 'yɔ̃ɔ sɛsɛbɛ pɔ, ka kɔkɔr yi be a Nãaŋmɩn puorfʋ yir a nãa dakɔɔ par 'yɛrɛ kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, "A maal naa!"
66016018	Be lɛ ka saa nyɩɩrfʋ, nɩ gɔ̃mɔ̃, nɩ saa tãnfʋ wa, ka a tẽe dam wʋ jaa miin kpɛ̃ɔ. An yi a lɛ daar jaa, nɩsaal na be ka a wɛr pɔ a tẽe ba mii a kpɛ̃ɔ a lɛ ɛ.
66016019	Ka a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ 'mar jiir ata, ka a paalsɩ tẽbɛrɛ mɩ lo lo. Nãaŋmɩn chɛnɛ na tɩɛr tɔ a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ Babilon na wʋ gbʋ̃m wʋ a dãa na sɛɛ ŋmele na ɩ a wʋ suur.
66016020	Dõdolsɩ a jaa bɔr naa ka fʋ kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ tɔ̃ɔ go ɛ,
66016021	ka a sakpʋlõbibɛrɛ na tɩrɛ yire a saaju loro ŋmiere a nɩbɛ ka ba tʋrɔ a Nãaŋmɩn a sakpʋlõbie gefʋ nyã jũu.
66017001	A malakasɩ ayopõi na tara a laar ayopõi, ɩ̃sʋɔ wan wa 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Wa, ɩn wiil fʋn a lɛ a pɔɔ baa nyã yuor na yi na jɩ̃nɛ a mansɩ nɛɛ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ.
66017002	'Lɔ lɛ a wɛr nãmɩne gãn ka a wɛr nɩbɛ mɩ buu nɩ a wʋ sɛ̃sɛ̃yele."
