66017003	Be lɛ, a malaka 'mɔɔ man a Sɩɛ pɔ chiin a mɔgɔ̃ɔ pɔ. Be lɛ n tɩ nyɛ a pɔɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a mɔdʋ̃jɩɛ ju. Ka a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nyã ɩ̃gãn wʋ jaa pɔɔn yoe na fere nɩ Nãaŋmɩn na wʋ tara jur ayopõi nɩ ɩlɛ pie.
66017004	A pɔɔ vaar naa fɔjɩ ile ile na wʋ pɩ̃ɛn sɛlma nɩ kʋsɩsʋ̃n nɩ lɛrbikpɩ̃ɛn. Wʋ tara naa a sɛlma ŋmele a wʋ nũsʋ̃ɔ pɔ a wʋ tʋ̃ kakaba nɩ a wʋ sɛ̃sɛ̃yele na sɛɛ.
66017005	Yuor sɛb mar a wʋ gberaa pɔ, "Fʋn kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ bɔ̃ɔ a par ɛ, a Babilon na yi yuor, pɔɔ baar ma, nɩ a wɛr tʋ̃ kakabsɩ ma."
66017006	N nyɛn a pɔɔ na nyũ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ jɩ̃ɩ buu, a bala na di a Yesu dãasɩɛ. Ɩn wa nyɛ wʋ a lɛ, nɛɛ 'maa ma naa.
66017007	Ka a malaka sʋʋr ma, "Ŋmɩnɛ a nɛɛ 'maa fʋ? Ɩn wiil fʋ naa a pɔɔ nɩ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ wʋn do na tara jur ayopõi nɩ ɩlɛ pie yelsɔɔlaa par.
66017008	A mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ fʋn nyɛ, wʋ dɔ̃ɔ be be, pʋ̃pãanyã waa lɛ be be go ɛ. Wʋn yi naa a bɔɔ fulom pɔ na wʋ chen a sɔ̃ɔfʋ jie. A wɛr nɩbɛ bala yoe na ba sɛb a nyɛvʋr gãn pɔ ɛ, yi a wɛr maalfʋ daar ɛ, bala wa nyɛ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nyã, nɛɛ na 'maa ba naa bojũu wʋ dɔ̃ɔ be be na waa lɛ be be ɛ, tɩ na wʋn lɩɛb wa.
66017009	"A ka ɩ naa tɩɛr na tara yɛ̃ 'yɛr. A jur ayopõi ɩ naa a tɔ̃n ayopõi a pɔɔ na jɩ̃nɛ, nɩ a nãmɩne ayopõi.
66017010	A ba anũu kpi naa tɩ ka bʋ̃'yen chɛnɛ, bʋ̃'yen mɩ ba wa sɛrɛ ɛ. Tɩchɛ 'lɔ wa wa, wʋn kor bɩ̃lãa.
66017011	A mɔdʋ̃ɔ 'lɔ na dɔ̃ɔ be be na waa lɛ be be go ɛ, wʋ ɩ naa a nãmɩne aniin sʋɔ na pʋɔ ayopõi bala pɔ na chiine a sɔ̃ɔfʋ jie.
66017012	"A ɩlɛ pie ala fʋn nyɛ ɩ naa nãmɩne pie na ba di a nãa sɛrɛ ɛ, tɩchɛ ban kʋ ban kpɛ̃ɔ ka ba ɩ nãmɩne lɔ̃ɔn a mɔdʋ̃ɔ sɔ̃ɔ bɩ̃lãa.
66017013	Ba jaa tɩɛr ɩn bʋ̃'yen, ka ba de a ba kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ fɔ̃ɔ kʋ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ.
66017014	Ban ŋmaan naa a Pɛraabile jɛɛr, tɩchɛ ka a Pɛraabile na tʋ̃ɔ ba, bojũu 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a sorbo ba jaa Soro nɩ a nãmɩne ba jaa Nãa. A bala wʋn bʋɔl na wʋ chɛl ir ka ba turo nɩ yelmɩ̃ɛ, na pʋɔ wʋ naa."
66017015	Ka a malaka 'yɛr kʋ ma, "A kɔ̃n ala fʋn nyɛ be a pɔɔ baa 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ, ɩ naa a nɩbʋrsɩ, nɩyɔɔ, paalsɩ nɩ 'yɛrbʋrsɩ.
66017016	A mɔdʋ̃ɔ nɩ a ɩlɛ pie ala fʋn nyɛ ban 'laar naa a pɔɔ baa nyãna na ba tɔɔ wʋ chɩɛr tɩ chɛ wʋ sal'mʋɔr. Ban 'wɔb wʋ naa tɩ chɛ 'yɔ̃ɔ bũu pɔ ka wʋ di.
66017017	Bojũu an ɩ Nãaŋmɩn lɛ de 'yɔ̃ɔ a ba tɩɛr pɔ ka ba na ɩ a wʋ bɔfʋ, ka ba jaa tɩɛr ɩ bʋ̃'yen ka ba sɔɔ de a ba kpɛ̃ɔ kʋ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ ka wʋ di nãa ka Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr wa maal baar.
66017018	A pɔɔ fʋn nyɛ ɩ naa a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ nãa na tʋ̃ɔ a wɛr nãmɩne ba jaa."
66018001	A anyã puor, n nyɛn a malaka ɩ̃sʋɔ na yi a saaju suro waara. Wʋ tara na kpɛ̃ɔ. A chãa na be a wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ chaar naa a wɛr wʋ jaa.
66018002	Na wʋ tãn kpɛ̃ɔ nɩ nɛkpɛ̃ɛ 'yɛrɛ, "Wʋ wɛl naa! A Babilon tẽkpɛ̃ɛ 'lɔ wʋ wɛl naa! Wʋ lɩɛb dɛɛr dẽme gaa jie, nɩ sɩdɛbɛ, nɩ lubil dɛbɛ nɩbɛ na ba ɔɔrɔ ɛ kpɛfʋ jie.
66018003	Bojũu an ɩ a paalsɩ ba jaa buu naa nɩ a wʋ sɛ̃sɛ̃yele, ka a nãmɩne na be ka a wɛr pɔ gãn wʋ. A yayarba na be a wɛr pɔ len tu a wʋ bʋ̃yɔɔ pɔ."
66018004	Be lɛ n lɛ wõ kɔkɔr ɩ̃sʋɔ na yi a saaju 'yɛr, "Maa nɩbɛ, yɩ wa yi a wʋ pɔ na yɩ taa ɩrɛ wa pʋɔ a wʋ dɛɛr pɔ ɛ, bɩɩ na yɩ pʋɔ a wʋ wõm pɔ ɛ.
66018005	Bojũu a wʋ maal dɛbɛ dɔɔl taa tɩ ta a saaju, ka Nãaŋmɩn tɩɛr tɔ a wʋ dɛɛr wʋn maal.
66018006	Yɩ kʋ wʋ nɩtãa lɛ wʋn kʋ yɩ. Yɩ yab wʋ tɩ lɛ dɔɔl wʋ. Yɩ kʋ wʋ a dãa nɩ a wʋ ŋmele nɛɛr ayi ka wʋ nyũ.
66018007	Ge wʋ ka wʋ waal, a yuor nɩ a nʋ̃ɔ wʋn bʋɔrɔ kʋrɔ a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ. Wʋ ma chɛn nyãa 'yɛr, 'N ɩn pɔɔ nãa jɩ̃nɛ, n ba ɩ pɔɔ kʋɔr ɛ. Nɩbaal kʋ̃ wa kpɛ ma jaa ɛ.'
66018008	A lɛ jũu, bɩbir bʋ̃'yen lɛ a wõm na wa a wʋ ju, kũu, nɩ kõn, nɩ kɔ̃. Bũu lɛ ɩ a di wʋ an ɩ a Soro Nãaŋmɩn nyã na tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr ɩn tʋ̃ɔfʋ sʋɔ.
66018009	"Ka a wɛr nãmɩne na dɔ̃ɔ gãn wʋ na ba 'mataa din wʋ a nʋ̃ɔ, bala wa nyɛ a lɛ wʋn dire ka a jʋʋr uro, an ɩrɛ ban nɩbaal ka ba kõnõ kʋrɔ wʋ.
66018010	Dãbɩ̃ɛ kpɛ ba naa a ger nyã jũu, ban ara na tɛɛr jaa tɩ kõnõ 'yɛrɛ, 'Nɛbier, nɛbier, a fʋ̃ʋ tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã, pa Babilon, a fʋ̃ʋ nyã na tara a kpɛ̃ɔ, bɩbir bʋ̃'yen lɛ a sɔ̃ɔfʋ be wa a fʋ ju.'
66018011	"A yayarba na be a wɛr pɔ na kõnõ na tɩ waala bojũu nɩrɛ ba be be na da a bonsɩ go ɛ.
66018012	A sɛlma, kpãna, kʋsɩsʋ̃n nɩ a lɛrbikpɩ̃ɛn, nɩ fuu pɩɛl, nɩ fuujɩ ile ile, nɩ fuu saalsɩ, nɩ a fuujɩ kpɩ̃n kpɩ̃n, nɩ a daar ala nyũu na nʋ̃mɔ̃, nɩ bomo ala jaa ban de wab chɛlɛ maal. A daar ala daa na be tuo, a kurjɩɛ, nɩ kursɔɔlɔ, nɩ a kʋsɩkpũlo bie.
66018013	A kãnyũu vɩɛl ala, nɩ a dãn, nɩ a kãn, nɩ a jɔ̃n, nɩ chir, nɩ a niin, nɩ a piir, nɩ a wiisɩ, nɩ a wiisɩ torkosɩ, nɩ a gbãgbaar.
66018014	"A bʋ̃vɩɛlsɩ ala na ɩrɛ fʋ a vɔlaa, a jaa chen naa. A fʋ nãbomo naa fʋ yobɔyele a jaa bɔr naa. Fʋ kʋ̃ lɛ nyãa go ɛ.
66018015	A yayarba na da a bomo kʋ wʋ na ba le, nɛɛ na 'maa ba naa a wʋ ge fʋ nyã pɔ, ka ba sɛr yi tɛɛr jaa tɩ kõnõ waala
66018016	'yɛrɛ nɩ, 'Nɛbier, nɛbier, a fʋ̃ʋ tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã, a fʋ̃ʋ na ma su a fɔpɩɛl, nɩ a fɔjɩ ile ile, nɩ a fɔkpɩ̃n kpɩ̃nsɩ. Na fʋ ma pɩ̃ɛn a sɛlma, nɩ a kʋsɩsʋ̃n, nɩ a lɛrbikpɩ̃ɛn.
66018017	Mɔ̃tɔ̃ bʋ̃'yen lɛ a fʋ nãbomo anyãna be wɛ a jaa.' A bala na kaara a gborbɛrɛ ala a man kpɛ̃ɛ pɔ, nɩ a nɩbɛ bala na be be, nɩ a bala jaa na tʋ̃nɔ̃ dire be a man pɔ, na ara na tɛɛr.
66018018	Bala wa nyɛ a jʋʋr ban kõnõ na 'yɛrɛ nɩ, 'Tẽbuor lɛ be ka na wʋ ta a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã?'
66018019	Ban ɔɔn tãna 'yɔ̃ɔnɔ̃ a jur pɔ tɩ kõnõ tɩ waala 'yɛrɛ nɩ, 'Nɛbier, nɛbier, a fʋ̃ʋ tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã. A jie nyã a bala jaa na tara a gborbɛrɛ yʋɔrɔ nɩ a man pɔ, ba jaa len tu a fʋ jie, tɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ bʋ̃'yen a fʋ be wɛ a nɩtɔ̃?'
66018020	Saaju, chɩlɛ a wʋ jũu, yɩn Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ nɩ a nɩtʋ̃nsɩ nɩ a 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ yɩ chɩlɛ. Nãaŋmɩn tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr nɩtãa a lɛ wʋn maal yɩ."
66018021	Be lɛ ka a malaka kpɛ̃ɔ pãa 'mɔɔ kʋsɩr kpɛ̃ɛ na jɩ̃tãan nɩɛr lɔb 'yɔ̃ɔ a man pɔ tɩ 'yɛr, "Nɩtɔ̃ lɛ ɩn lɔb fʋ bar, a fʋ̃ʋ Babilon tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã ka nɩrɛ kʋ̃ lɛ nyɛ fʋ jaa go ɛ.
66018022	Ba kʋ̃ lɛ wõ kõrõjom ŋmefʋ, nɩ yiel yielbe, nɩ daa pɛɛlbɛ, nɩ ɩlɛ pɛɛlbɛ jaa go ɛ. Tʋ̃tʋ̃nbɔ jaa bʋrɔ kʋ̃ lɛ be be go ɛ, ba kʋ̃ lɛ wõ jɔ̃ nɩ̃ɛnbɛ dɔ̃ɔn go ɛ.
66018023	Fɩ̃tɩn bũu kʋ̃ lɛ chaar be go ɛ. Ba kʋ̃ lɛ wõ pɔɔ paalaa nɩ wʋ sɩrɛ kɔkɔr go ɛ. A fʋ yayarba lɛ dɔ̃ɔ yi yuor a wɛr pɔ. A fʋ tɩ̃sɔɔ yele lɛ fʋ de bɛl a paalsɩ jaa ka ba bɔr.
66018024	A wʋ pɔ lɛ ba nyɛ a 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ jɩ̃ɩ nɩ bala ba jaa ban dɔ̃ɔ kʋ a wɛr pɔ."
66019001	A anyã puor, n wõn gɔ̃mɔ̃ fɩka nɩyɔɔ na tãna be a saaju 'yɛrɛ nɩ, "Dãnfʋ wʋ ta Nãaŋmɩn! Faafʋ nɩ tɩɩr nɩ kpɛ̃ɔ ɩ naa a wʋ tʋɔr,
66019002	bojũu a wʋ 'yɛr tɔɔrfʋ ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ tɩ mɩ tor. Wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔn a pɔɔ baa na 'yɛr, 'lɔ lɛ sɔ̃ɔ a wɛr nɩbɛ nɩ a wʋ sɛ̃sɛ̃yele. A wʋ gbãgbaar wʋn kʋ, wʋ yab wʋn a sãn."
66019003	Ba lɛ tãna na go, "Dãnfʋ wʋ ta Nãaŋmɩn. A wʋ jʋʋr na uro duoro ba tara ŋmaafʋ ɛ."
66019004	Ka a nɩbɛrɛ lɩjɛr nɩ anaar nɩ a bʋ̃nɩbie anaar bala gãn kpa tẽe puor a Nãaŋmɩn na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju pɛɛrɛ wʋ 'yɛrɛ nɩ, "A ɩ a lɛ. Dãnfʋ wʋ ta a Nãaŋmɩn."
66019005	Be lɛ ka a kɔkɔr yi be a nãa dakɔɔ par 'yɛrɛ, "A yɩn na ɩ a Nãaŋmɩn gbãgbaar na yɩ joro wʋ dãbɩ̃ɛ. Ka bil bɩɩ bɛrɛ lɛ, yɩ pɛɛrɛ a sɩ Nãaŋmɩn!"
66019006	N pãa lɛ wõn dɔ̃ɔn fɩka nɩyɔɔ na gɔ̃nɔ̃, bɩɩ fɩka kɔ̃kpɛ̃ɛ na joro, bɩɩ saa na tãna kpɛ̃ɔ jaa, "Dãnfʋ wʋ ta Nãaŋmɩn! Bojũu a sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ, lɛ di a nãa.
66019007	Yɩ ɩ a sɩ chɩlɛ ka sɩ ɩ̃gãn 'maa a sɩ kʋ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr an ɩ a wʋ Pɛraabile pɔɔ kulfʋ bɩbir vɩɛ naa, ka a pɔɔ mɩ chɔɔr a wʋ mɩ̃ɛ baar.
66019008	Wʋ sun bʋ̃pɩɛl na vɩɛlɛ tɩ nyɩlɛ." A bʋ̃pɩɛl anyãna lɛ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ yeltorsɩ.
66019009	Ka a malaka 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Sɛb a anyãna, 'An ɩn pʋpɛl kʋ a bala ban bʋɔl a Pɛraabile pɔɔ kulfʋ lɔ̃ɔ di jie.' " Ka a malaka mɩ 'yɛr pʋɔ, "A Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr anyãna ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ."
66019010	Ka n gã kpa tẽe ɩka n puor wʋ, tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Ta maal a lɛ ɛ. N mɩ ɩ naa a gbãgbaa nɩtãa a fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a fʋ yɛɛr kaar, bala lɛ tara Yesu dãasɩɛ. Puor Nãaŋmɩn! Bojũu, a Yesu dãasɩɛ lɛ ɩ a Sɩɛ 'yɛr."
66019011	N nyɛn a saaju na yuo, ka a ɩ wii pɩla lɛ, ka a nɩrɛ 'lɔ na do yuor di, yelmɩ̃ɛ sʋɔ nɩ nɩtor. Yeltorsɩ lɛ wʋ ma tɔɔr a wʋ 'yɛr tɩ ŋmaan wʋ jɛɛr.
66019012	A wʋ nɩbie 'lɩrɛ naa fɩka bũu, ka a nãjupil yɔɔ su a wʋ ju pɔ. Yuor sɛb mar wʋ nɩrɛ jaa na ba bɔ̃ɔ ɛ, ka 'lɔ tɛɛ ba lɛ ɛ.
66019013	A fuu wõo wʋn su ɩn jɩ̃ɩ wʋ jaa ka a yuor di, "Nãaŋmɩn 'Yɛr."
66019014	A saaju sojasɩ sun bʋ̃pɩɛl don wii pɩɛl turo nɩ wʋ.
66019015	Ka a sɔkpɛ̃ɛ diir yi a wʋ nɛɛ pɔ, 'lɔ lɛ wʋ de chɩɛrɛ nɩ a paalsɩ ba jaa, "Wʋn kaara ba jaa nɩ a kpɛ̃ɔ 'lɔ na kaara a kur dãgbal kaar." Wʋn nɛɛrɛ ban ŋmɛrɛ be a tɩɛ wɔ̃mɔ̃ nɛŋmɛrfʋ jie nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ a Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ suur.
66019016	Yuor nyãna lɛ be a wʋ fuu wõo na suu a gbɛkpɛ̃ɛ pɔ ɩka, A NÃMƖNE BA JAA NÃA, NƖ A SORBO BA JAA SORO.
66019017	N nyɛn malaka na ara a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ ju tɩ bʋɔl a lubil a jaa na ɔɔrɔ be a saaju nɩ kɔkɔkpɛ̃ɛ, "Yɩ lɔ̃ɔ taa wa a Nãaŋmɩn lɔ̃ɔ di jie.
66019018	Lɛ lɛ, yɩ wa dire a nãmɩne ɩ̃gãma nɩ a fɔ̃n dẽme nɩ a kpɩ̃ɛn dẽme, a wiisɩ nɩ a ba duorbo, gbãgbaar nɩ sumɩne, a bil nɩ a bɛrɛ, a nɩbɛ banyãna ba jaa ɩ̃gãma."
66019019	Ka n nyɛ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nɩ a wɛr nãmɩne nɩ a ba sojasɩ lɔ̃ɔn taa ŋmaan a 'lɔ na do a wii nɩ a wʋ sojasɩ jɛɛr.
66019020	Tɩchɛ ba nyɔɔn a mɔdʋ̃ɔ lɔ̃ɔn a jir ŋmara 'yɛ'yɛrɛ na tʋ̃ a nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ niem. A nɛ'maa tʋ̃mɔ̃ anyãna lɛ wʋ de bɛlʋ̃ a bala na tara a mɔdʋ̃ɔ jɩ̃nɛ tɩ puor a bʋtɩɩ. Ba lɔb ba jaa ayi bʋ̃nɩbie 'yɔ̃ɔ a jerbɩ bũu na dire pɔ.
66019021	A bala na chɛ, a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a wii ju kʋ ba naa nɩ a sɔkpɛ̃ɛ diir 'lɔ na yi a wʋ nɛɛ pɔ, ka a lubil pãa di a ba ɩ̃gãma tɩɩ.
66020001	N nyɛn a malaka na yi a saaju suro waara tara a bɔɔ fulom 'lɔ pãn bir nɩ bɔ̃jɔr gbor.
66020002	Wʋ tʋ̃ɔ naa a dajɩl 'lɔ na ɩ a kõr waa, 'lɔ lɛ ɩ a dɛɛr sʋɔ na ɩ a Satan na wʋ lũ wʋ nɩ a bɔ̃jɔr gbor ka wʋ̃n maal yuomo tur (1,000).
66020003	Wʋ lɔb wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ a bɔɔ fulom nyã pɔ, tɩ kpal na wʋ 'yɔ̃ɔ jɩ̃nɛ a wʋ kʋ̃ lɛ tʋ̃ɔ a paalsɩ bɛl go ɛ, ka a yuomo tur (1,000) wa baar. A ala puor, ban yuo wʋ naa ka wʋ maal ber bɩ̃lãa.
66020004	N nyɛn nãa dakɔɔr, ka a bala na jɩ̃nɛ, ba kʋ ban sɔr ɩka ba tɔɔr 'yɛr. N lɛ nyɛ naa a bala na dɔ̃ɔ dire a Yesu dãasɩɛ nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn 'yɛr jũu ban kʋ, n nyɛn a ba sɩɩr. Bala lɛ ba sɔɔ puor a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nɩ a bʋtɩɩ ɛ, bɩɩ sɔɔ de a wʋ jɩ̃nɛ a ba gber pɔ bɩɩ a nuur pɔ ɛ. Ba ir naa a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋɛ ka bala naa Yesu lɔ̃ɔ di nãa a yuomo tur (1,000).
66020005	A kũn bala na chɛ baa ir ɛ, ka a yuomo tur (1,000) ala ba wa baar ɛ. A dɔ̃ɔ dɔ̃ɔ kũu pɔ irfʋ lɛ a anyã.
66020006	Pʋpɛl lɛ kʋ a nɩ chɛchɛsɩ banyãna na de nie ir a kũu pɔ ɩ vʋɛ. A gbɛɛ ayi kũu kʋ̃ lɛ pɔɔ ba go ɛ, tɩchɛ ban ɩn a Nãaŋmɩn bɔɔr lorbo, ka bala nɩ a Nɩ-iraa lɔ̃ɔ di nãa a yuomo tur (1,000) ala pɔ.
66020007	A yuomo tur wa ta, a malaka na yuo naa a Satan a bɔɔ fulom 'lɔ pɔ na wʋ for wʋ bar,
66020008	ka wʋ yi bɛlʋ̃ a wɛr kõkobo anaar wʋ jaa nɩbɛ, Gɔɔg nɩ Magɔgɩ na wʋ lɔ̃ɔ ba jaa ka ba ŋmaa jɛɛr. A nɩbɛ waa naa fʋn kʋ̃ tʋ̃ɔ ba sɔr ɛ.
66020009	Ba yɛr a wɛr wʋ jaa na ba wa jilʋ̃ a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ jaa jie a tẽe 'lɔ a Nãaŋmɩn na nʋ̃. Tɩchɛ ka a bũu yi saaju lo di ba jaa.
66020010	Ka a dɛɛr sʋɔ 'lɔ na bɛlʋ̃ ba, ba lɔb wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ a jerbɩ bũu na dire pɔ, be lɛ a mɔdʋ̃ɔ nɩ a jir ŋmara 'yɛ'yɛrɛ be. Ban ge ba naa mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ nɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ wʋ jaa, ka ba be be jaa kpo kpo.
66020011	N pãa lɛ nyɛn a nãa dakɔɔ pɩla, ka a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ. A tẽe nɩ a saaju bɔr a wʋ niem, baa lɛ tara jie go ɛ.
66020012	N nyɛn a kũn, bil naa bɛrɛ ka ba ara a nãa dakɔɔ niem, a ba yuor gãma bin. Ba lɛ yuon a gãn ɩ̃sʋɔ na ɩ a nyɛvʋr gãn. Ba tɔɔr naa a kũn bala 'yɛr nɩtãa a lɛ ban dɔ̃ɔ maal a ba sɛb 'yɔ̃ɔ a gãn pɔ bin.
66020013	A man tɩr naa a kũn ala wʋn tara, ka a kũu nɩ a kpĩisɩ tẽe mɩ tɩr a kũn bala ban tara, ka ba tɔɔr nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa 'yɛr a lɛ wʋn dɔ̃ɔ maal.
66020014	Ba lɔb a kũu nɩ a kpĩisɩ tẽe 'yɔ̃ɔ a bũu dagel pɔ. A bũu nyã na dire lɛ a kũu gbɛɛ ayi.
66020015	Ala ɩ nɩrɛ jaa yuor ba wa sɛb a be a nyɛvʋr gãn pɔ ɛ, ban lɔb wʋn 'yɔ̃ɔ a bũu dagel nyã pɔ.
66021001	A anyã puor, n pãa nyɛn saaju paalaa nɩ tẽpaalaa, bojũu a saaju koraa nyã nɩ a tẽkoraa nyã bɔr naa, ka a man ba lɛ be be go ɛ.
66021002	N nyɛn a Tẽchɛchɛ na ɩ a Jerusalɛm paalaa ka wʋ yi a saaju a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ suro waara fɩka, pɔɔsaraa na pɩ̃ɛn bʋ̃kãkaɛ gun a sɩrɛ kulfʋ.
66021003	Ka n wõ kɔkɔr na yi a be a nãa dakɔɔ par 'yɛrɛ, "Pʋ̃pãanyã, Nãaŋmɩn na kpɩɛraa a nɩsaalba pɔ, na wʋ be a ba sɛ̃. Ban ɩn a wʋ nɩbɛ, ka wʋ mɩ be a ba sɛ̃ ɩ a ba Nãaŋmɩn.
66021004	Wʋn 'yɩɛr naa a ba nɩbikʋ̃ɔ a nie pɔ bar. Kũu kʋ̃ lɛ be be go ɛ. Waal ba lɛ be be go ɛ. Kõn mɩ ba lɛ be be go ɛ. Nɩrɛ ba lɛ bɩɛrɛ be go ɛ. Bojũu a yelkoro a jaa põn chen."
66021005	Ka a 'lɔ na jɩ̃nɛ a nãa dakɔɔ ju 'yɛr, "N maala naa a bomo a jaa bʋ̃paalaa!" Na wʋ pãa lɛ 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Sɛb a anyãna bin, baal ba be be ɛ, a ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ."
66021006	Wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ma, "A maal naa. Maa lɛ a Pielfʋ nɩ a Baaraa. 'Lɔ jaa a kɔ̃nyũur na kpɛ, ɩn kʋ wʋn a nyɛvʋr kʋ̃ɔ na yi a bulo pɔ ka wʋ nyũ pɔrɔ.
66021007	Nɩrɛ 'lɔ jaa na jɛb tʋ̃ɔ, ɩn kʋ wʋn a anyãna a jaa. Ka n ɩ a wʋ Nãaŋmɩn ka wʋ mɩ ɩ a n bie.
66021008	Tɩchɛ a bala na ɩ a dãbɩ̃n dẽme, nɩ bala na ba sɔɔ de ɛ, nɩ tɩɛr dɛbɛ dẽme, nɩ nɩkʋrbɔ, nɩ sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ, nɩ sʋɔbɔsɩ, nɩ tɩpuorbo, nɩ jir ŋmarba ba jaa, a ba jie ɩ naa be a jerbɩ bũu dagel pɔ. A nyã lɛ ɩ a kũu gbɛɛ ayi."
66021009	Ka a malakasɩ ayopõi na tara a wõm ayopõi 'lɔ na tara a baaraa wa 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Wa, ka n wiil fʋ a pɔɔsaraa na ɩ a Pɛraabile pɔɔ."
66021010	A malaka 'mɔɔ man a Sɩɛ pɔ don a tɔ̃ wõo kpɛ̃ɛ ju na wʋ tɩ wiil ma a Tẽchɛchɛ na ɩ a Jerusalɛm na yi a Nãaŋmɩn sɛ̃ suro waara.
66021011	Wʋ chaar wʋ jaa nɩ a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr, a chaarfʋ kaara fɩka a kʋsɩsʋ̃n na wʋ nyɩlɛ chaar jaa wel wel a kʋsɩbɛ ala ban bʋɔlɔ a jasɩpa kaar.
66021012	Dachin wõo na kpɛ̃mɛ jilʋ̃ wʋ jaa na wʋ tara dɔ̃dɔɩ pie nɩ ayi, ka a dɔ̃dɔr ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa tara malaka na kaara. Ba sɛb a Isɩral bal pie nɩ ayi yoe mar a dɔ̃dɔɩ pɔ.
66021013	Dɔ̃dɔɩ ata ben a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ purfʋ jie, ka ata mɩ be a kõkoor, ka ata mɩ be a kõkoor nyã, ka a ata mɩ be a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ mʋrfʋ jie.
66021014	Dachin par kparsɩ pie nɩ ayi ju lɛ a dachin dɔɔl. Ala pɔ lɛ ba sɛb a Pɛraabile nɩtʋ̃nsɩ pie nɩ ayi yoe dɔɔl.
66021015	A malaka 'lɔ na 'yɛrɛ nɩ ma tara na sɛlma damanaa ɩka wʋ man a tẽe dɔ̃dɔɩ nɩ a dachin.
66021016	A tẽe par kparaa jɩ̃taa, a wõofʋ nɩ a yalfʋ wʋ jaa. Wʋ man a tẽe nyɛ ka wʋ ɩ mɛl tur dɔɔl kɔɔr anaar (1,400). A wõofʋ nɩ a yalfʋ, a dofʋ, nɩ a jãafʋ.
66021017	Wʋ man a dachin ka a yal ɩ gbɛɛ kɔɔr ayi dɔɔl pie nɩ ayʋɔb (216). A malaka man a lɛ a nɩsaal na ma man.
66021018	A kʋsɩbɛ ala ban bʋɔlɔ a jasɩpa lɛ ba mɛn a dachin, ka a tẽe wʋ jaa ɩ sɛlma na wʋ chaar chãana kaar.
66021019	Kʋsɩsʋ̃n a jaa bʋrɔ lɛ ba de kpar a tẽe par kparaa. A par kpardɔ̃ɔ 'lɔ ɩn a kʋsɩsʋ̃n ala ban bʋɔlɔ a jasɩpa, ka a ayi sʋɔ mɩ di safer, ka a ata sʋɔ di agete, ka a anaar sʋɔ mɩ di ɛmerald,
66021020	ka a anũu sʋɔ di ɔnɩksɩ, ka a ayʋɔb sʋɔ mɩ di kanɩlian, ka a ayopõi sʋɔ di keresolɩtɩ, ka a aniin sʋɔ mɩ di berl, ka a pie forbir sʋɔ di topajɩ, ka a pie sʋɔ di kɩrɩsopɩrase, ka a pie nɩ bʋ̃'yen di jasɩntɩ, ka a pie nɩ ayi sʋɔ mɩ di amɛtesete.
66021021	A dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ pie nɩ ayi ala ɩ naa a kʋsɩsʋ̃n pie nɩ ayi. Kʋsɩbʋ̃'yen lɛ ba maal a jaa. A sɔkpɛ̃ɛ na be a tẽkpɛ̃ɛ nyã pɔ sɛlma lɛ wʋ jaa ka wʋ chaar chãana kaar.
66021022	N ba nyɛ puorfʋ yir be a tẽe pɔ ɛ, bojũu a sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ɩ Tʋ̃ɔfʋ Sʋɔ nɩ a Pɛraabile lɛ ɩ a puorfʋ yir.
66021023	A tẽe nyã ba bʋɔrɔ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ, bɩɩ ŋmɛraa chãa ɛ, bojũu a Nãaŋmɩn tɩɩr lɛ ɩ a chãa, ka a Pɛraabile ɩ a wʋ fɩ̃tɩn.
66021024	A chãa nyã pɔ lɛ a paal bʋrsɩ nɩbɛ na yʋɔrɔ, ka a wɛr nãmɩne mɩ waan a ba nãbomo a be.
66021025	A wʋ dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ ba be na wa pɔɔ a mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ ɛ, an ɩ tɩ̃sɔɔ ba lɛ be be go ɛ.
66021026	A paal bʋrsɩ nɩbɛ nãbomo nɩ a ba tɩɩr, ban waan naa be.
66021027	Bʋ̃dɛɛr kʋ̃ kpɛ be ɛ, bɩɩ bala na tʋ̃nɔ̃ vĩ tʋ̃mɔ̃, bɩɩ nɩbɛlbɛ, tɩchɛ a bala tɛɛ yuor na sɛb a Pɛraabile nyɛvʋr gãn pɔ.
66022001	Ka a malaka pãa wiil ma a nyɛvʋr põn kʋ̃ɔ ka wʋ ɩ jaa wel wel ka a joro yire a Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Pɛraabile nãa dakɔɔ par,
66022002	naa joro a tẽe sɔr kpɛ̃ɛ sãlsɔɔ. Nyɛvʋr tɩɛ ara naa a põn lõbobo, ka a jaa ma wɔ̃nɔ̃ wɔ̃bʋrsɩ pie nɩ ayi yuon jaa, ka a wiil ɩka a ma wɔ̃ naa ŋmɛraa jaa gbɛbʋ̃'yen. A vaɩ lɛ ban sãan a paalsɩ a jaa nɩbɛ baal.
66022003	Nãaŋmɩn pɔ'yɔ̃ɔfʋ ba lɛ be bon jaa pɔ go ɛ. Nãaŋmɩn nɩ a Pɛraabile nãa dakɔɔ na ben a tẽe pɔ, ka a wʋ gbãgbaar tʋ̃nɔ̃ kʋrɔ wʋ.
66022004	Ban nyɛn a wʋ nie, ka a wʋ yuor be a ba gber pɔ.
66022005	Tɩ̃sɔɔ kʋ̃ lɛ be be go ɛ. Baa lɛ bʋɔrɔ fɩ̃tɩn chãa ɛ, bɩɩ mɔ̃tɔ̃ɔ chãa ɛ. Bojũu a sɩ Soro Nãaŋmɩn mɩ̃ɛ na chaar ba naa a wʋ chãa, na ba di nãa bɩbir jaa.
66022006	Ka a malaka 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Baal ba be a 'yɛrbie anyãna pɔ ɛ, a ɩn yelmɩ̃ɛ. A Soro Nãaŋmɩn na ma kʋ a wʋ Sɩɛ a wʋ 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ tʋ̃ naa a wʋ malaka ɩka wʋ wa wiil a wʋ gbãgbaa yele ala na kʋ̃ yaar tɩ ɩ ɛ."
66022007	"Nyɛ, n kʋ̃ yaar tɩ wa ɛ! Pʋpɛl sʋɔ lɛ a 'lɔ na sɔɔ a 'yɛrbie anyãna a jaa na sɛb a gãn nyã pɔ."
66022008	Maa Jɔɔn lɛ wõ tɩ nyɛ a anyãna. Ɩn wa wõ tɩ nyɛ a lɛ baar, n gãn kpa tẽe ɩka n puor a malaka, 'lɔ lɛ wile ma a anyãna.
66022009	Tɩchɛ ka wʋ 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Ta maal a lɛ ɛ! N mɩ ɩ naa a gbãgbaa nɩtãa a fʋ̃ʋ nɩ a fʋ yɛɛr 'yɛ'yɛrbɛ nɩ bala jaa na turo a gãn nyã 'yɛr. Puor Nãaŋmɩn!"
66022010	Ka a malaka pãa 'yɛr kʋ ma, "Ta sɔɔl a 'yɛ'yɛrɛ 'yɛr nyãna a gãn nyãna pɔ bar ɛ, bojũu a sɔ̃ɔ gbʋr naa.
66022011	Vɛ̃ ka a 'lɔ na ɩ nɩdɛɛr, wʋ chɛnɛ ɩrɛ a dɛɛr. Vɛ̃ ka a 'lɔ mɩ na maala yeldɛbɛ, ka wʋ chɛnɛ maala a yeldɛbɛ. Vɛ̃ ka a 'lɔ na tor, wʋ chɛnɛ ɩ a nɩtor. 'Lɔ mɩ na ɩ chɛchɛ, wʋ chɛnɛ ɩ a chɛchɛ."
66022012	"Nyɛ, n kʋ̃ yaar tɩ wa ɛ! N tara na a n yar na kʋ nɩrɛ jaa lɛ wʋn tʋ̃.
66022013	Maa lɛ a Pielfʋ nɩ a Baaraa, a nidɔ̃ɔn nɩ a puor sʋɔ.
66022014	"Pʋpɛl dẽme lɛ a bala na pɛɛ a ba fuusɩ. Ban tara na sɔr di a nyɛvʋr tɩɛ wɔ̃mɔ̃, na ba tu a dɔ̃dɔr nɛɛ kpɛ a tẽe pɔ.
66022015	Tɩchɛ baar, nɩ a sʋɔbɔsɩ, nɩ a sɛ̃sɛ̃nbɛ, nɩ a nɩkʋrbɔ, nɩ a tɩpuorbo, nɩ a bala jaa na nʋ̃ jir ŋmaafʋ, ban ara na a yõo.
66022016	"Maa Yesu lɛ tʋ̃ a n malaka nɩ a dãasɩɛ nyãna a yɩ sɛ̃ kʋ a pupuorbiir gbulsɩ. Maa lɛ ɩ a David nyɩɩr nɩ a wʋ yɔ̃ɔ, nɩ a bivɩɛ ŋmɛrbir na chaar."
66022017	Ka a Sɩɛ nɩ a pɔɔ paalaa 'yɛr, "Wa!" Ka a 'lɔ mɩ na wõ naa 'yɛr, "Wa!" Nɩrɛ jaa kɔ̃nyũur na kpɛ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ wa, nɩrɛ jaa na bʋɔrɔ, vɛ̃ ka wʋ wa de a nyɛvʋr kʋ̃ɔ kʋfʋ nyũ pɔrɔ.
66022018	N kpãan ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa na wõnõ a 'yɛ'yɛrɛ 'yɛr a gãn nyãna pɔ. Ala ɩ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa wa den bon dɔɔl a 'yɛr nyã pɔ, Nãaŋmɩn mɩ na dɔɔl wʋ naa a wõm ala a gãn nyã na 'yɛr a ba 'yɛr.
66022019	Ka ala ɩ nɩrɛ ɩ̃sʋɔ jaa mɩ wa ir bon bar a 'yɛ'yɛrɛ 'yɛr a gãn nyã pɔ bar, Nãaŋmɩn mɩ na mɔ̃ɔ wʋ naa a nyɛvʋr tɩɛ wɔ̃mɔ̃ nɩ a tẽchɛchɛ pɔ kpɛfʋ a gãn nyã na 'yɛr a wʋ 'yɛr.
66022020	A 'lɔ na di a anyãna dãasɩɛ 'yɛr naa, "Ɔ̃ɔ, n kʋ̃ yaar tɩ wa ɛ." A ɩ a lɛ. Wa sɩ Soro Yesu.
66022021	A sɩ Soro Yesu wɩ̃ɛfʋ wʋ be a Nãaŋmɩn nɩbɛ sɛ̃. A ɩ a lɛ.
